40001001	Thɩ kɔ̃ ʋrɛraakɛ Jeju Kirisitikɛ dɔnɩ Davɩdɩɩ bi məl, Abɩrahamɩ məl thenɩ.
40001002	Abɩraham kɔɔ kɔna Ɩjkɩ dɩ Ɩjakɩ kɔ̃ Jakɔbɩ, dɩ Jakɔbɩ gba kɔ̃ Juda na ɔɔ õkuunsɔ;
40001003	dɩ Juda gba kɔ̃ Farɛsɩ na Jara khɛr ʋrɛraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Tamaar, dɩ Farɛsɩra kɔna Ɛsɩrɔm, dɩ Ɛsɩrɔm gba kɔ̃ Aram;
40001004	dɩ Aram kɔ̃ Amɩnadabɩ, dɩ Amɩnadabɩ gba kɔ̃ Nasɔ̃, dɩ Nasɔ̃ gba kɔ̃ Salmɔ̃;
40001005	dɩ Salmɔ̃ gba kɔ̃ Boajɩ khɛr ʋrɛraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Rahabɩ, dɩ Boajɩ gba kɔ̃ Obɛɛdɩ khɛr ʋrɛraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Ruti;
40001006	dɩ Obɛɛdɩ kɔ̃ Ɩjaɩ, dɩ Ɩjaɩ gba kɔ̃ Davɩdɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ fãgadaar. Dɩ Davɩdɩ gba kɔ̃ Salomɔ̃ khɛrraakɛ kɔɔ dɔnɩ Urii khɛr;
40001007	dɩ Salomɔ̃ gba kɔ̃ Roboam, dɩ Roboam gba kɔ̃ Abɩa, dɩ Abɩa gba kɔ̃ Aja;
40001008	dɩ Aja gba kɔ̃ Jojafatɩ, dɩ Jojafatɩ gba kɔ̃ Joram, sɩ Ojɩasɩ dor Joramɩ məl;
40001009	dɩ Ojɩasɩ gba kɔ̃ Joatam, dɩ Joatam gba kɔ̃ Akaajɩ, dɩ Akaajɩ gba kɔ̃ Ejekɩasɩ;
40001010	dɩ Ejekɩasɩ gba kɔ̃ Manase, dɩ Manase gba kɔ̃ Amɔ̃, dɩ Amɔ̃ gba kɔ̃ Jojɩasɩ;
40001011	dɩ Jojɩasɩ gba kɔ̃ Jekonɩasɩ na ɔɔ õkuunsɔ, bɔɔkɛ wɩ fʋlɛnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldara a jalna Babɩlɔn.
40001012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ fʋlɛnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldara a jalna Babɩlɔn pɩ, gɛr Jekonɩasɩ kɔɔ kʋɔn Salatɩɛl, dɩ Salatɩɛl gba kɔ̃ Jorobabɛl;
40001013	dɩ Jorobabɛl gba kɔ̃ Abiyudi, dɩ Abiyudi gba kɔ̃ Elɩakɩm, dɩ Elɩakɩm gba kɔ̃ Ajɔɔr;
40001014	dɩ Ajɔɔr gba kɔ̃ Sadɔkɩ, dɩ Sadɔkɩ gba kɔ̃ Akɩm, dɩ Akɩm gba kɔ̃ Eliyudi;
40001015	dɩ Eliyudi gba kɔ̃ Eleajaar, dɩ Eleajaar gba kɔ̃ Matã, dɩ Matã gba kɔ̃ Jakɔbɩ;
40001016	dɩ Jakɔbɩ gba kɔ̃ Jojɛfɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Marɩɩ ko, Marɩɩkɛra kɔɔ kɔnanɩ Jejuukɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Kirisiti.
40001017	A fʋna Abɩrahamɩ bɔɔ a dana Davɩdɩɩ bɔɔ, thɩ kʋɔn yʋɔr yenã haanle fɛʋ; dɩ a fʋna Davɩdɩɩ bɔɔ a dana bɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ fʋlɛnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldara a jalna Babɩlɔn, thɩ kʋɔn yʋɔr yenã haanle, dɩ a fʋna bɔɔkɛ wɩ fʋlɛnɩ Ɩjɩryɛldara a jalna Babɩlɔn a dana Kirisitii bɔɔ, thɩ kʋɔn yʋɔr yenã haanle.
40001018	Hɩnɛ mɔ̃ gɩ kɔɔ danɩ sɩ dɩ wɩ kɔ̃ Jeju Kirisiti. Jojɛfɩ kɔɔ wɛna Jejuu nɩ Marɩ, sɩ wa kɔɔ dã kha pa', sɩ Thu Phuu cʋgɛɛ dɩ hana pɛmɛr.
40001019	Sɩ gɩdonɩ ɔɔ ko Jojɛfɩ dor tɩɩ sarʋ, aa ƴaal a kʋɛsʋʋ ire tibil jɔra ga, sɩ ɔɔ hara a kpɩɛr sa yɩ ɩna fagʋʋrɛ gbulu.
40001020	Dɩ hɩnɛ, mɔ̃ a hanɩ ga kpɩɛraalera, Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl pʋɔraarɛ dəəlela a sʋʋraa: Jojɛfɩ, Davɩdɩɩ bikuun, fa-n do maar n fʋ fɩ afɩ khɛr Marɩɩ kpara ga, gɩdonɩ pɛmɛrɩlera a hananɩ Thu Phuu pa gɩ the.
40001021	Kũubir a na kɔ̃ dɩ fa dʋʋ ire Jeju, gɩdonɩ ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ na taanɩ ɔɔ too awɩ sopugosɔra.
40001022	Gɩrɛ fɛʋ daan, gɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ gbanɩ ɔɔ bobonɩ nɔ a mɩɩna gɩ ha oti, gɩ sor:
40001023	“Hɩnɛ, khɛ biireekɛ na jɛnɩ kuun pa', a na hananɛ pɛmɛr a na kɔ̃ kũubir, wɩ haa ire Emanʋɛl”, i kɩrʋ dʋɔn Thãgba har kha na sɛrɛ.
40001024	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jojɛfɩra jaanɩ, a cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurə sʋʋraanɩ, dɩ a kpar ɔɔ khɛrra a kɔna,
40001025	sɩ aa-n phɩnaa ga, phaphapha dɩ kɔ̃ kũubirrə a haa irera Jeju.
40002001	Bɛtɩlɛhɛm Jude dɩɩra wɩ kɔɔ kɔ̃ Jeju, dɩ dabɔɔlera Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ do fãgadaar. Dɩ hɩnɛ, tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔɔkɛ jɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ ƴepələ̃berə kɔɔ ther kɩrrɔ a pɔ dã Jerujalɛm,
40002002	dɩ wa-n bule ayɩ: Juifisɔɔ fãgadaarɩkɛ wɩ kɔnɩ, kana a ha? Gɩdonɩ ɔɔ ƴepələ̃bi sɩ kɔɔ yɩ kɩrrɔ a ɩ̃ sɩ fʋɔrʋʋ.
40002003	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar nɩɛnɩ gele, ɔɔ kpɩɛr nyanyaanɛ na wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanaanɩ kha le Jerujalɛm.
40002004	Dɩ a kpar bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna fɛʋ nakha tɩbɩlaa jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaarsɔ, a bule wi ka teananɩ wɩ kɔna Kirisitira.
40002005	Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Bɛtɩlɛhɛm Jude dɩɩra gɩ, gɩdonɩ gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobon kɔɔ kherenɩ, gɩ sor ayɩ:
40002006	“Fɛr Bɛtɩlɛhɛmɩkɛ dɔnɩ Juda dɩɩ, sobɔr gɩ, fa do dɩɩkɛ 'lunoni a jɔ Juda dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔa'. Gɩdonɩ afɩ pa kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ na thɔɔnɩ mɛr Thãgbaa tookɛ dɔnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldara na the.”
40002007	Le Ɛrɔɔdɩ wolõ a we tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔ, a jɩɩ bule wi a jɩɩ jɩ bɔɔbɔɔ bɔɔkɛ ƴepələ̃bireelera phanɩ.
40002008	Agɩpɩ dɩ thɔ̃ wɩ Bɛtɩlɛhɛm dɩɩra ayɩ: Nɩ jala a jɩɛ 'lo bɩsaanɩdaalera; ado nɩ yɩɩ, nɩ dɔ ɩ̃ nɩɛ ɩ̃ jal dakha mer ɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋ.
40002009	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ gelela fãgadaarɩle so warnɩ pɩ, wɩ jaal. Dɩ hɩnɛ, ƴepələ̃bireekɛ wɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ kɩrrɔ, ɔr kʋlɛ wɩ ƴɩɛ a jal phaphapha a dã ka bɩsaanna hanɩ a jɩɩl ƴũ.
40002010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩnɩ ƴepələ̃bireele, da kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ kɔɔ fʋ wɛr na sobɔr.
40002011	Dɩ wɩ pɔ dã a lõ cʋɔrɔɔlera a yɩ bɩsã buurə nakha ɔɔ nɩ Marɩ, dɩ wɩ gburõkure a fʋɔrʋʋ, sɩ agɩpɩ, wɩ thʋbɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ wɩ pɔnanɩ a haa khaardaa, dɛ gɩ na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnanɩ daʋ, nakha thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hɔnɩ latɩkolo ni caar.
40002012	Sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ mɩɩna wɛr dəəlela wa-n bir jal Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ pa bã, dɩ wɩ bire gba hʋ kpɩɩ a kɔ̃ awɩ dʋɔ.
40002013	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔ kɔnɩ pɩ, hɩnɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl pɔr Jojɛfɩra dəəlela a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Ɩrɛ, gba biikɛra na ɔɔ nɩ, a fuo jala Ejipiti, a tɔɔ le gɩ dana bɔɔkɛ ma so farnɩ fɩ kɛr fɩ ɩ̃, gɩdonɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ n ƴaalɛ a kʋ biikɛra.
40002014	Dɩ Jojɛfɩ ɩɩr dɩtɩnɔna, a gba biile na ɔɔ nɩ a jal Ejipiti.
40002015	Dɩ le a too phaphapha Ɛrɔɔdɩ khinə, dɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛɛkɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ gbanɩ ɔɔ bobonɩ nɔ a mɩɩna dã otirə, gɩ sor: “Mɛr Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ wɛ ɩ̃ Bikuun dɩ the Ejipiti.”
40002016	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ yɩnɩ mɔ̃ kpɛsɛsɔɔle fɩɩlʋʋnɩ, nĩkhii fʋʋrɛ dɩɩ pho ka, dɩ hɩɩnɔ bɔɔkɛ tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔ kɔɔ mɩɛnɩ, sa thɔ̃ Bɛtɩlɛhɛm dɩ bɩnɔ na Bɛtɩlɛhɛm dɩ khuirə fɛʋ, a kʋʋr bɩsã kuuminə fɛʋ phaphapha a jalna dana yɛna yenyɔdara.
40002017	Dɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobon Jeremɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ dã a ha oti, gɩ sor:
40002018	“Hulẽbe kɔɔ ther Rama, khɩsa na benɩɛ jɔɔ. Rasɛl gɩ da-n bɩ ɔɔ bɩsãsɔra. A bor ayɩ, ɩna faa haara', gɩdonɩ wa hale bã.”
40002019	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ khini pɩ, hɩnɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl bire pɔ Jojɛfɩra Ejipiti, a sʋʋraa dəəlela ayɩ:
40002020	Ɩrɛ, gba biikɛra na ɔɔ nɩ a kɛra birə Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩra, gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n kɔɔ ƴaalɛnɩ bɩsã buukɛraa yʋ wɩ khiire.
40002021	Dɩ Jojɛfɩ ɩɩr a gba bɩsã buurə na ɔɔ nɩ a kɛr bir Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩra.
40002022	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ Arkɛlayʋsɩ kɔɔ gbaan ɔɔ thɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ too pa a do fãgadaar Jude dɩɩra, maar fʋʋrɛ, aa 'la na lõ la', sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ mɩɩnaanɛ dəəlela, dɩ kɛr jal lõ Galile khʋra,
40002023	a pɔ too dɩ bɩɛllaakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Najarɛtɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ na dã oti, gɩ sor: “Wa-n wɩɩrɛ Najarɛtɩdaar.”
40003001	Ga bɔɔlera Jã Batɩsɩtɩ ɩɩr da-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Jude bəənnə da-n so ayɩ:
40003002	Nɩ deba haar, gɩdonɩ bɔɔ daan dɩ ƴũ Eãgadaar na-n gba fãga.
40003003	Jana dɔ ʋrɛ Ejaɩ Thãgbaa bobon kɔɔ sonɩ ayɩ: “Tibil wire gɩ dɩ ga-n hulẽ bəənnə ayɩ: Na-n gbɛbɩrɛ hʋɛ Kɔ̃tɩnna, na-n wɛbɩrɛ ɔɔ hʋ bisɔ gɩ pɔlɔ.”
40003004	Kɩ̃kɩɩnɩkɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ nyɔɔmɛɛ sũu Jana n kɔɔ to, dɩ khɩmɩna lo phɛrɛ pelela. Sɩ toosõo na thʋʋr n kɔɔ dɔ ɔɔ dɩko.
40003005	Dɩ Jerujalɛmdara na Judedara fɛʋ, na wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ thɛnɩ Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩr khʋra, n kɔɔ pɔr ɔɔ pa,
40003006	dɩ wɩ cã awɩ sopugosɔ, sɩ da-n kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔ Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩrra.
40003007	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ a yɩnɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala', dɩ wa-n pʋɔraa jɔɔjɔɔ a kpɛa wɩ nyʋɔnɔ, a so warɛ ayɩ: Nɛr sikori bisɔ, amɛ sɔ nar nɩ fuo Thãgbaa nĩkhirəəkɛ na ɩnanɩ?
40003008	Na-n sɛ beekɛ n nɛnanɩ anɩ ha debi.
40003009	Na-n too na kpɩɛr anɩ hara waa ayɩ, Abɩraham dʋɔn anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tã', gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ dɩ bokanaakɛrakɛ Thãgba punone a cʋʋ gɩ dɩ gɩ debi a do bɩsana Abɩrahamna.
40003010	Dɩrakɛ kpãkpo 'lire leere thɩr nɛ kuur leere, dɩ thɩrʋ wo thɩrʋʋkɛ na-n sɛnɩ bi bʋɔa', wa kurre na dʋna dɔɔ.
40003011	Me wer nyʋɔnɔ mɩ-n kpɛɛ nɩ dɩ na debi haar, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na kpaanɛnɩ, a hananɛ fãga a jɔ mɩ, dɩ ma hɩɩrʋʋrakɛ a na julẽ ɔɔ nɛfaa ga. Ɔr, Thu Phuurə na dɔɔra a na kpɛɛ nɩ.
40003012	Dɩ jʋ jɛ nyɔ̃kpʋʋn hale dɩ fʋrɔ ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ. A na jɛr jɔ a gba jʋ be a pɛ ɔɔ thʋ̃ bɩnɔ, sɩ a thii laagbee dɔɔraakɛ na dɔnɩ thɩ̃ khiirnənə'.
40003013	Ga bɔɔlera Jeju the Galile, a pɔ Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩrra Jãa pa a kpɛa nɩ nyʋɔnɔ.
40003014	Sɩ Jã kɔɔ bor sa so ayɩ: Mɛr ka teena fɩ kpɛa mɩ nyʋɔnɔ, sɩ dɩ fɩ ka ɩ̃ marɩ?
40003015	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Nɛnɛ̃ wer, sɛ gar gɩ ha mɛ̃. Gɩdonɩ gɩ teenanɛ dɩ sa cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ saranɩ. Dɩ Jã na kɔɔ banaa bã.
40003016	Dɩ dapaara ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kpɛɛnɩ Jeju nyʋɔnɔ dɩ na the, hɩnɛ thãgbara ƴũ phubire dɩ yɩ Thãgbaa Thu da-n gbũ a ho puusɩ̃ɛ a pɔ lʋʋnaa.
40003017	Dɩ hɩnɛ, nʋɔ ther le thãgbara ƴunə a so ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, a lõ mer haar kpɛ.
40004001	Agɩpɩ Thu Phuu thɔɔ Jeju a jalna bəənnə Satã n fifilənee.
40004002	A kɔɔ lire nʋɔ a cʋʋna wire kpalanyɔ na dɩtɩnɛ kpalanyɔ, agɩpɩ kɔmɛr fʋʋrɛ.
40004003	Dɩ fifilədaarɩlera tɔr dã a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Ado Thãgbaa Bikuun fɩ do, sɔ bokananaakɛ gɩ debi gɩ do dɩkor.
40004004	Sɩ dɩ Jeju birsee: Gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Ga do dɩkor dɩbara na hana tibil yirə', sɩ thɩmɩa fɛʋʋkɛ n thɛnɩ Thãgbaa nɔra gɩ.”
40004005	Agɩpɩ dɩ Satana bir kpaa a jalna dɩ phuurəəkɛ dɔnɩ Jerujalɛm, a jʋʋnna Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna ƴũ, sa sʋʋraa:
40004006	Ado Thãgbaa Bikuun fɩ do, ubo je thʋnɔ, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere ayɩ: “Thãgba na pɛrɛ ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ wɩ tɛ fɩ, a mɛ̃ gaa fa ber nɔɔ bokaarra.”
40004007	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Gɩ kherere dakha wo ayɩ: “Fa-n fifilə Kɔ̃tɩn afɩ Thãgba a hɩɩna'.”
40004008	Dɩ Satã kpaa wo a jalna jʋʋnna gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ gbaanɔnɩ dɩɩ ka, a nɩɩraa fãgadaar dɩɩsɔ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ thɩɩra na awɩ nyɔ̃kor bɔ,
40004009	sa sʋʋraa: Fɛr ma ha thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛra ado fa gburõkure na fʋɔr mɩ.
40004010	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Hala jala pal Satã. Mee gɩ kherere ayɩ: “Kɔ̃tɩn afɩ Thãgba fa fʋɔr, dɩ ɔrra dɩbara fa doro thɔma.”
40004011	Agɩpɩ Satã sɩɩraa, dɩ hɩnɛ, Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ pɔr dɩ wa-n haa gɩrɛ n danaanɩ.
40004012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ fʋrɛ Jã a to khaɩra, a kɛrrɛ bir lõ Galile.
40004013	Mɛ̃ a the Najarɛtɩ dɩɩra a jal too Kapɛrnayʋm mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔra Jabʋlɔ̃ na Nɛfɩtalɩ bəənnə.
40004014	Gɩ do mɛ̃ gɩrɛ Ejaɩ Thãgbaa bobon sonɩ dã oti, gɩ sor:
40004015	“Jabʋlɔ̃ dɩɩ na Nɛfɩtalɩ dɩɩ, mɩɩr nɔ hʋɛ, kɛ hanɩ Jʋrdɛ̃ iiro, Galile ca kpala.
40004016	Tɩbɩlaakɛ hanɩ dabirəra, wɩ yɩrɛ dahɩrɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, na wɩrɛɛkɛ hanɩ khĩdi dɩ birəra, dahɩrɛ carã warɛ.”
40004017	A fʋna ga bɔɔlera Jeju ma da-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ dɩ yɩ: Nɩ deba haar, gɩdonɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ bɔ daan.
40004018	Mɔ̃ Jeju n jalnɩ na Galile mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔ, a yɩrɛ õkona yenyɔ, Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pɩɛr gɩ, na Ãdire ɔɔ õkuun, dɩ wa-n dʋna thʋ̃ pherdaakɛ n hɔnɩ jɔ̃ lanyʋɔnɔ, gɩdonɩ thʋ̃ pherdara ha wɩ.
40004019	Dɩ a so warɛ: Na-n kpa mar, dɩ ma cʋʋ nɛr na-n ƴaal tɩbɩla thʋ̃ khaa.
40004020	Dɩ dapaara, wɩ faarɛ awɩ thʋ̃ pherdasɔ sɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
40004021	Dɩ bir tɔ na jal wo a yɩ wɩ̃ õkona yenyɔ, Jakɩ Jebedee bikuun, na Jã ɔɔ õkuun, dɩ wɩ ha kha na awɩ thɩ Jebede gboroona, dɩ wa-n gbɛbɩ awɩ thʋ̃ pherdasɔ.
40004022	Dɩ a we wer, dɩ dapaara wɩ faarɛ gborõo na awɩ thɩ sɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
40004023	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ kpaarɛ Galile dɩɩra fɛʋ, da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ, da-n mɩɩna tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ ƴũ fãgadaar doda, da-n kpɛɛna khoosɔ dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ, na tãdarasɔ dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
40004024	Dɩ ɔɔ i kpaarɛ Siri dɩɩra fɛʋ. Dɩ wɩ kpar wɩrɛɛkɛ kho caar dɩɩdɩɩ fʋnɩ dɩ wa-n gaar, na wɩrɛɛkɛ n 'wãganɛnɩ: Kpãkpũdara, na ji khidara, na gbãgbarasɔ a pɔnanaa dɩ a kpɛɛ wɛr.
40004025	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ ther Galile, na Dekapol, na Jerujalɛm, na Jude, na Jʋrdɛ̃ iiro dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
40005001	Mɔ̃ Jeju yɩnɩ tibil jɔjʋɔɔle, a jʋʋnɛ gɔ̃gʋɔna ƴũ a too, dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara tɔr a wɔrɔ̃ɔ.
40005002	Agɩpɩ dɩ ma da-n dɩɩr wɩ thakɛ ayɩwɔɔ:
40005003	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ jɩɛnnɩ dɩ thu thɩ̃ɛ n ɓɔr wɛr, gɩdonɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ wɛr hɩna.
40005004	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ n bɩɛnnɩ, gɩdonɩ Thãgba na cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wa faa haar.
40005005	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ hɛlɛlɛ fɩldara, gɩdonɩ wɛr na hɩna thɩɩkɛ.
40005006	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛnɩ gɩrɛ saranɩɩ cʋʋra, gɩdonɩ Thãgba na cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wa 'li dɩbara.
40005007	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ n dɔnanɩ tɩbɩla bʋɔ, gɩdonɩ wɛr Thãgba na dona bʋɔ.
40005008	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ hananɩ ha phuu, gɩdonɩ wɛr na yɛ Thãgba.
40005009	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ n cʋɛnɩ ha ɩɩ dɩ ga-n hale, gɩdonɩ wɛr wa-n we Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔ.
40005010	Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ wɩ-n kpooronɩ dɩɩ do fɩl sarʋ dɔ nɔɔ, gɩdonɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ wɛr hɩna.
40005011	Gɩ da nar ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n nɩɩr nɩnɩ dɩ wa-n kpoona nar, dɩ wa-n kʋɛna anɩ isɔ na sõso bɩɩ, dɩɩ do mɛr dɔ nɔɔ, gɩdonɩ mɛ̃ wɩ kɔɔ kpoo Thãgbaa bobonasɔraakɛ kɔɔ kʋlɛ nɩnɩ ƴɩɛ.
40005012	Nɩ dɔ daʋ na-n fʋ nɩ na-n kãka, gɩdonɩ anɩ khaardaakɛ na 'lɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, ga kɔ̃tɩnɛ.
40005013	Nɛr dʋɔn laan thɩɩra, sɩ ado laan bir dasɩ a mɩla bã, mɔ̃ wa fʋ sɩ na cʋʋ gɩ dɩ ga bir na hana mɩlalɛ? Ga dor ga bɔr bã, khuirə wa dʋna na faa mɛ̃, dɩ tɩbɩla na-n saar na nɛɛ.
40005014	Nɛr dʋɔn dahɩrɛ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ thɩɩra. Dɩɩkɛ wɩ thenɩ gɔ̃gʋɔna na puno na kera'.
40005015	Dɩ wa-n pɛ dɔɔ lãphana a suuro bɩlãkpʋʋnna', sɩ bilela wɩ-n dɛ̃ɛ dɩɩ hɩrɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩle cɔ bɩnɔ.
40005016	Nɩ dɔ anɩ dahɩrɛ na-n hɩrɛ tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra thale, wɩ puno wa-n yɩ anɩ thɔ̃ bɔsɔ, wa-n dʋbɩ anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũu i.
40005017	Na-n kpɩɛr waa mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ kʋkʋʋl Thãgbaa jɔfʋa', dɩ Thãgbaa bobonaa so ga. Ma ɩ̃ ɩ̃ kʋkʋʋl ga, sɩ ɩ̃ ka ɩ̃ cʋʋ gɩrɛ fɛʋ jɔfʋ n ƴaalnɩ ga-n cʋɛ.
40005018	Gɩdonɩ sobɔr mɩ so nar, a fʋna bɔɔkɛ ƴũ na thɩɩ hanɩle na jalna na pɩna, dɩkhaa thɩ̃ bu fɩɩʋ na halerakɛ jɔfʋra gɩ do gɩ kʋkʋʋla', foo thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ n cʋʋ gɩ dã oti.
40005019	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na kʋɛanɩ jɔfʋsɔɔkɛ bɩɛl, a jɔfʋ buu gɩrakɛ fɩɩʋ dɩ ntɛ kʋɛ, sɩ da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla wa-n cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃, ɔr wa we dabuu ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n hɩnɛ gɩnɩ sɩ da-n dɩɩrna tɩbɩla wa-n cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃, ntɛɛle wa-n we kɔ̃tɩn ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
40005020	Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ, ado anɩ fɩl sar na ba jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔɔda ga, na lõ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra yuuraka'.
40005021	Nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ wɩ kɔɔ sonɩ mamadarara ayɩ: “Fa-n kʋ tibilə'.” Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kɔnɩ tibil, a na 'lɛr kɩɩlɛ.
40005022	Sɩ me wer mɩ so narɛ gɩrɛ: Tibil wo tibilikɛ nĩkhi haar, kɛ na fʋnɩnakɛ ɔɔ omina, a na 'lɛr kɩɩlɛ. Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na nɩrɛnɩ ɔɔ omi, gɩ daan dɩ wa kɩɩlnaa Juifi so gʋʋrdaraa ƴɛra, dɩ ʋrɛ na sɔnɩ ɔɔ omina nayɩ, də̃bəl haa, gɩ daan dɩ ntɛɛle na jal bu paar dɔɔra.
40005023	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ado fɩ-n 'laarɛ khaardaa Thãgba fʋɔr paar dɩɩ do le fɩ jɩnanɛ afɩ omi hananɛ sor na fɛrɛ,
40005024	faa le afɩ khaarda Thãgba fʋɔr paar sa jala nɩ gʋʋr kha sor na afɩ omi ɓo gɩ pɩ, sɩ fɩ bir fɩ jal fɩ 'laa afɩ khaarda dɩphã.
40005025	Nɩ kuune kha kɔrɔ na afɩ sodaar, bɔɔkɛ nɩ hanɩ kha hʋɛra dɩ na-n jal. Agado mɛ̃ gaa, afɩ sodaar na gba fɛr na ha so kɩɩldaar, dɩ so kɩɩldaar na gba fɩ dakha na ha gardɩ, dɩ gardɩ na gba fɩ na to khaɩra.
40005026	Sobɔr mɩ so far, fa the liir kpɩɩraka', phaphapha fɩ lɩmɩ afɩ mũsũ koo fɩ pɩ.
40005027	Nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ wɩ so ayɩ: “Fa-n ƴaal khɛ kpɩa', fa-n ƴaal kuun kpɩa'.”
40005028	Sɩ me wer mɩ so narɛ gɩrɛ: Tibil wo tibilikɛ n hɩnɛnɩ khɛr ƴaƴaal hɩɩnʋ, gɩ dor a ƴaalɛ khɛrɩle le ɔɔ hara a pɩ.
40005029	Ado afɩ nyɔ̃bɔ yi do far baradaa, te dɔna faa ƴɔɔ, gɩdonɩ ga ba farɛ ado afɩ tomɩ ɓã bɩɛl bu, gɩ baar gɩrɛ wa gbanɩ afɩ tomɩ koo na dʋna bu paar dɔɔra.
40005030	Ado afɩ nyɔ̃bɔ nyɔ̃ do farɛ baradaa, kuro dɔna faa ƴɔɔ, gɩdonɩ ga ba farɛ ado afɩ tomɩ ɓã bɩɛl bu, gɩ baar gɩrɛ wa gbanɩ afɩ tomɩ koo na dʋna bu paar dɔɔra.
40005031	Gɩ kɔɔ sor dakha ayɩ: “Ado ntɛ na faa ɔɔ khɛr a hanaa he kuur sɛbɛ.”
40005032	Sɩ me wer mɩ so narɛ: Tibil wo tibilikɛ na faanɩ ɔɔ khɛr, sɩ agado kũu kpɩɩ ƴaalɛ dɔ nɔa', gɩ nɩnanɛ a cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ debi do kũu kpɩɩ ƴaaldaar, dɩ tibilikɛ na hɛnɩ khɛrɩkɛ wɩ faanɩ, khɛ ƴaal kpɩɩ sopugo a cʋʋ.
40005033	Nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ wɩ kɔɔ so wo mamadarara ayɩ: “Fa-n ʋlfɛ sõso ʋlfɛra', sɩ cʋɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ fɩ kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ Kɔ̃tɩn.”
40005034	Sɩ me wer mɩ so narɛ: Na-n ʋlfɛ kpɩɩraka', dɩ na-n ʋlfɛrakɛ na Thãgbaa dʋɔa', gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa fãga too pa gɩ.
40005035	Na-n ʋlfɛ na thɩa', gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa nɛ jəəda gɩ, na-n ʋlfɛ na Jerujalɛm dɩa', gɩdonɩ Fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dɩ gɩ.
40005036	Fa-n ʋlfɛ na afɩ yʋa', gɩdonɩ fa punonakɛ na cʋʋ afɩ yʋsũ bɩɛllakɛ dɩ ga bulolo, agɩbo gɩ biiroə'.
40005037	Ado nɩ so thɩ̃ɛ ayɩ, ɔɔ, nɩ dɔ gɩ do ɔɔra; anɩ ooho n do oohora, gɩrɛ na hanɩle na ɓaan, ga dor puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩ pa gɩ the dɩphã mɛ̃.
40005038	Nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ wɩ kɔɔ so ayɩ: “A tibil kʋɛ tibil yire, wɩ kʋɛaa yire dakha. A nyɩnɛ a khaa, wɩ khaa nyɩnɛ dakha.”
40005039	Sɩ me wer mɩ so narɛ: Na-n kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ kha na tɩɩ puə'. A tibil ka ɓa fɩ nyɔ̃bɔ gbʋaa, birə fe gbʋa kpɩɩ pɩɛraa wo.
40005040	A tibil ƴaal ɩnɩ-n wɛ fɩ kɩɩl paar a gba fɩ kẽkẽ gburo, birə gba afɩ darã a ɓananaa.
40005041	A tibil tɔ fɩ na fãga pɛr nɩ jala kha gɩ dã kilə bɩɛl, tɔ kilə bɩɛl pɩɛr gɩ ha yenyɔ.
40005042	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n bɩɛlnɛ farnɩ thɩ̃ɛ hanaa, fa-n tɔ̃ ʋrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ a pemi far thɩ̃a'.
40005043	Nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ wɩ kɔɔ so ayɩ: “Fa-n na afɩ 'walãkha tibil,” sɩ na laarɛ afɩ lãlaardaar.
40005044	Sɩ me wer mɩ so narɛ: Na-n na anɩ lãlaardara, na-n bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba na pɛ wɩrɛraakɛ n kpoa narnɩ.
40005045	Thale na do bɩsana anɩ Thɩraakɛ hanɩle ƴũ, gɩdonɩ a-n cʋʋrɛ ɔɔ wi dɩɩ phã tɩɩ puusɔra na tɩɩ bɔɩsɔra, dɩ cʋʋ dakha nyʋɔn dɩ ga-n dã tɩɩ sarasɔra na wɩrɛra na sarana'.
40005046	Gɩdonɩ ado nɩ-n nar wɩrɛɛkɛ n naan nɩnɩ, anyee khaarda na 'lɛ? Ga do thalera war gbadara n cʋʋ dakha gaa?
40005047	Dɩ ado anɩ omi ha nɩ-n fʋɔr dɩbara, anye nɩ cʋʋ dɩɩ tiro a ha kpɩɩ? Ga do thalera wɩrɛ na jɛnɩ Thãgba ga n cʋʋ dakha gaa?
40005048	Gɛr gɩ nɛrɛ nɩ bʋɔnɔ a ka, mɔ̃kɛ anɩ Thɩ le ƴũ bɔrnɩ a ka.
40006001	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ na-n nɩna anɩ bɔ cʋʋ tɩbɩlala wa-n yɛ ga, a gɩ ha mɛ̃ na 'lɛ khaardaa anɩ Thɩraakɛ hanɩle ƴũ fɩɩʋraka'.
40006002	Gɛr gɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ-n hanɩ bɔdara thɩ̃ɛ, fa-n do wɩ ʋ̃ tutuu afɩ ƴɛra, mɔ̃kɛ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara n cʋʋnɩ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔa', na ƴatɔɔ tɩbɩla n yɛ wɩ a na khɩa wa'. Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wɩ 'lɛr awɩ khaarda thalera pɩ.
40006003	Sɩ fɛrɛ̃, ado fɩ-n har bɔdara thɩ̃ɛ, fa-n dorakɛ afɩ nyɔ̃bɩlã n jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ afɩ nyɔ̃bɔ n cʋʋna';
40006004	gɩ do mɛ̃ afɩ thɩ̃ 'laa na wolone, dɩ afɩ Thɩɩkɛra yɛ gɩnɩ wolonena ɔr na ka fɩ.
40006005	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba, na-n ho bɩnɛ yenyɔdaraakɛ n naannɩ ɩnɩ-n jɩlɛ na bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ na hʋ nʋɔrasɔ tɩbɩla na-n yɛ na'. Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wɩ 'lɛr awɩ khaarda thalera pɩ.
40006006	Sɩ fɛrɛ, ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba, lona afɩ du bɩnɔ a khaanɛ loo, sa bɩɛlnɛ afɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ ka keranɩ; dɩ afɩ Thɩɩkɛra n yɛnɩ gɩrɛ keranɩ, ɔr na ka fɩ.
40006007	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba, na-n ther thɩmɩa pɛrɛ pɛrɛ a na pɛra', mɔ̃kɛ thɩldara n cʋʋna', gɩdonɩ wɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ jɔ mɩɩrɛ na dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ Thãgba na tu awɩ bɩɛl.
40006008	Na-n ho waa koe, gɩdonɩ anɩ Thɩ jɩrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ n ɓɔra nɩnɩ, sɩ dɩ na kɔɔ bɩɛlɛɛ pa'.
40006009	Dɩ gɛr gɩ nɩ bɩɛlnɛ thakɛ: Asɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũ, dɔ afɩ i n dʋbɩrɔ;
40006010	dɔ afɩ fãgadaar do n ɩ̃; dɔ afɩ tuur na-n cʋʋ kɛ thɩɩra, mɔ̃ gɩ-n cʋʋɩɩɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
40006011	Hana sɩ nĩ dɩkorɩkɛ na dana sɩnɩ.
40006012	Faa asɩ puukɛ sɩ-n cʋʋnɩ na hana sɩ mɔ̃ sɛrɛ dakha n faanɩ ɩkhasɔɔ puukɛ wɩ-n cʋʋ sarnɩ dɩ sa-n ha wɩ.
40006013	Fa-n faa sɩ fifiləle n puno sa', sɩ na taa sɩ puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ. [Gɩdonɩ fɛr hɩna nũfiire, na punone, na i dʋbɩrɛ bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr. Amɛn.]
40006014	Dɩ ado nɩ-n faarɛ sopugookɛ tɩbɩla n cʋʋ narnɩ dɩ na-n ha wɩ, anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ ƴũ a na faarɛ anɩ sopugo dakha a na-n ha nɩ.
40006015	Sɩ ado na-n faa sopugookɛ tɩbɩla n cʋʋ narna', anɩ Thɩ na faa dakha anɩ sopugo na ha na'.
40006016	Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n lin nʋɔ, na-n ho bɩnɛ yenyɔdaraakɛ n lenɩ sɩ dɩ wa-n kpaar na gbobira', gɩdonɩ wɩ-n lire ƴɩɛ dɩ wa-n nɩna tɩbɩla wɩ jɛ nʋɔ ɩnɩ li. Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wɩ 'lɛr awɩ khaarda thalera pɩ.
40006017	Sɩ fɛrɛ, ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ-n lini nʋɔ, hulo ƴɩƴ, a bʋlana niin yʋʋ;
40006018	dɩ mɛ̃ fa nɩ̃na tɩbɩla wɩ jɩ nʋɔ fɩ lə', sɩ afɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ ka keranɩ ɔr fa nɩna, dɩ afɩ Thɩɩkɛra n yɛnɩ dakha gɩrɛ keranɩ, ɔr na ka fɩ.
40006019	Na-n khɩɩ lẽle thɩ̃ɛ a thɩɩn kɛ thɩɩra, ka ɔphãkerẽsɔ na dʋʋn na kʋɛ gɩna', na ka yo na cɩnɩ na cu sɩ na lõ na yuə'.
40006020	Sɩ na-n khɩa lẽle thɩ̃ɛ a na thɩnɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, kãkɛ ɔphãkerẽsɔ na dʋʋn na kʋɛ gɩna', dɩ yo wɛ a na cɩ na cu sɩ na lõ na yuə'.
40006021	Gɩdonɩ kãkɛ afɩ lẽle thɩ̃sɔ hanɩ, le afɩ ha na ha dakha.
40006022	Yire dʋɔn lãphã tormrra. Ado afɩ yi bɔr, afɩ tomɩ fɛʋ dahɩrɛra ga ha.
40006023	Sɩ adõ afɩ yi na bɔra', afɩ tõmɩ fɛʋ na har dabɩrəra. Sɩ ado dahɩrɛɛkɛ fɩ hananɩ afɩ bɩnɔ birəre, ga dor dabirəra na kɔtɩnɛ na ka.
40006024	Tibil bɩɛllakɛ na puno na do thɔma kɔ̃tɩna yenyɔra ga, foo a na laarɛ bɩɛl sɩ a na na bɩɛl, agɩbo a na mar kha an bɩɛl sɩ a hɛbɩ bɩɛl. Na puno na do thɔma Thãgbara nakha lẽle thɩ̃a'.
40006025	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so nar: Na-n too na dɛna anɩ yi gɩrɛraakɛ na khonɩ na-n yɔna ga, dɩ anɩ tomɩda gɩ gɩrɛraakɛ na tona'. Yire na ba dɩkoraa? Dɩ tomɩr na ba kɩ̃kɩɩnaa?
40006026	Nɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃kɛ 'lominə jɩɛra hanɩ. Wa-n diirə', wa-n kha ga, wa-n hana thɩ̃ɛ a ur thʋnɛna ga, sɩ anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ ƴũ, ɔr n haanɛ wɩ. Anɩ the nɔ ga khɩɩr a jɔ wɛr fĩiəə?
40006027	Ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil nɛrɛra dɛr na do nɔɔ da puno na dɛɛnɔ ɔɔ yɛ nɔ?
40006028	Dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n dɛ kẽkẽ thɩmɩɩrra? Na-n kpɩɛrna naporsɔ hʋɔnɔ wo na hɩnɛ mɔ̃ wɩ-n phuni. Wa-n do thɔma ga, wa-n kpar kẽkẽ wiirə'.
40006029	Sɩ mɩ so narɛ Salomɔ̃ɔ thɛthɛrakɛ, kɛ dɔnɩ fãgadaar, na ɔɔ nyɔ̃kor bɔ fɛʋ na kɔɔ to kɩ̃kɩɩn dɩɩ hona wɛr bɩɛllaka'.
40006030	Dɩ ado Thãgba na to hʋɔnɩkɛ hanɩle hʋɔnɔ nĩ dɩɩ ha thaa, sɩɩ do cʋɔ wa to garɛ dɔɔ, a na ka na cʋʋ mɛ̃ dakha nɛrɛraakɛ kanɩ hana ha pɛrɛ gbəə?
40006031	Dɩ gɛr gɩ na-n ha na dɛ a na so: Anye sa kho yaa, na anye sa yɔ yaa, agɩbo anye sa gba na to yaa ga.
40006032	Gɩdonɩ gelesɔ fɛʋ wɩrɛ na jɛnɩ Thãgba ga n ƴaalɛ gɩ. Sɩ anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũ, a jɩrɛ gɩrɛ n ɓɔra nɩnɩ.
40006033	Sɩ caca thɩ̃ɛ nɩ ka na ƴaalɛ ɓo Thãgbaa fãgadaar do na ɔɔ fɩl sar, sɩ gelesɔɔlerarakɛ fɛʋ Thãgba na ha nɛr a na ɓaan.
40006034	Dɩ gɛr gɩ na-n ha na dɛna cʋɔdaa ga, gɩdonɩ cʋɔɔ thɛthɛrakɛ n dɛnanɛ ɔɔbara. Na-n bãbanɛ na nĩkɛɛ nɩ, gɩ daan.
40007001	Na-n fi do kɩɩldara ga, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba na do nar Kɩɩldaara'. Mɔ̃ nɩ fi nɩ do kɩɩldara, mɛ̃ Thãgba na do nar Kɩɩldaar.
40007002	Gɩdonɩ mɩɛda ca ʋrɛ nɩ-n kɔɔ mɩɛnanɩ thɩ̃ɛ, ɔr wa mɩɛna na ha nɩ.
40007003	Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fɩ ka gar yire hɔ̃ phɩɩnaakɛ hanɩ afɩ omii yiro, sɩ fa-n ka dɩ fɩ hɩɩn kparrɛɛkɛ hanɩ afɩ yiroə?
40007004	Wo mɔ̃ fa fʋ sɩ na so afɩ omina nayɩ: Jɩlɛ ɩ̃ ti hɔ̃ phɩ̃ɩkɛ ha fɩnɩ yiro, sɩɩ dorakɛ kparrɛ hale afɩ yiro?
40007005	Fɛr bɩnɛ yenyɔdaar, te kparrɛɛkɛ hanɩ afɩ yiro ɓo, le fa jɩɩ yɩ hɔ̃ phɩ̃ɩkɛ hanɩ afɩ omii yiro dɩphã a na ti.
40007006	Na-n gba Thãgbaa thɩ̃ a na ha bena ga, anaa wa kɛrna fɛr a na cɛcɛbɛ fɩ. Na-n gba dakha anɩ dɛ thɩ̃ a na dʋna sɩthɔra ga, anaa wa bɩɩrnanɛ thɩɩ.
40007007	Na-n bɩɛlnɛ na 'lɛr, na-n ƴaalɛ na yɩɛrɛ, na-n bɛ loo wa khɛr nɛr.
40007008	Gɩdonɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n bɩɛlnɛnɩ a-n 'lɛr, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ a-n yɩɛrɛ, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n bɛnɩ loo wa khɛrʋʋrɛ.
40007009	Ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn ɔɔ bi na bɩɛllɔ buru dɩ na haa bokaar?
40007010	A thʋm a bɩɛl a haa sii?
40007011	Ado nɛrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ tɩɩ puusɔ jɩ thɩ̃ bʋɔ a na ha anɩ bisɔ, mɔ̃ ga thʋ̃ na da anɩ Thɩraakɛ hanɩle ƴũ na pɔna, a na gba thɩ̃ bʋɔ na ha wɩrɛɛkɛ n bɩɛlnɛnaa?
40007012	Thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nɩ-n ƴaalnɩ tɩbɩla na-n cʋɛ nar, nɛrɛ dakha na-n cʋɛ ga thɩ̃ ca wɛrra, gɩdonɩ gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ na Thãgbaa bobonaa so sonɩ.
40007013	Na-n lona na lõfonʋɔɔkɛ 'luruneni fɩɩʋ, gɩdonɩ lõfonɔ pɩɛ hə̃ə na hʋ pɩɛ hə̃ə dʋɔn gɩrɛ n jalananɩ bu paar, dɩ wɩrɛ kɛ harɔnɩ wɩ jɔrɛ ka.
40007014	Sɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ yɛnɩ lõfonʋɔɔkɛ 'luruneni ka, na hʋɛɛkɛ hanɩ ɓɩnɩnɩnɩ kɛ n jalanɩ yire khorra, wa kpɛra'.
40007015	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ sõso bobonasɔra, wɩ-n debire a ho banaasɔ a na pɔ anɩ pa, sɩ awɩ bɩnɔ kpe wɛ, kɛ n phʋnɛnɩ.
40007016	Sɩ awɩ biikɛ wɩ-n senɩ na jɩna wɩ. Fa khʋnɛ ɓãɓar be ʋsɩɛra ya? Dɩ fa yɛɛrɛ bara dakha pabɩrʋra ya?
40007017	Thale gɩ, thɩrʋ wo thɩrʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ thɩr bʋɔ, bi bɔɩra a-n se, dɩ thɩr puu na-n se bi puu oti.
40007018	Thɩr bʋɔ na puno na se bi puə', dɩ thɩr puu na puno na se bi bʋɔ dakha ga.
40007019	Dɩ thɩrʋ wo thɩrʋʋkɛ na-n sɛnɩ bi bʋɔa', wa kurre na dʋna dɔɔra.
40007020	Dɩ gɛr gɩ awɩ birəəkɛ wɩ-n senɩ na jɩ wɩ.
40007021	Ga do wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n wɛ mɩnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn, Kɔ̃tɩn, na lona ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra ga, sɩ ʋrɛ dɩbara n cʋɛnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũu tuur.
40007022	Tibil jɔjʋɔ na so marɛ dawiile nayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, Kɔ̃tɩn, ga do afɩ i sɩ kɔɔ gba dɩ sa-n tinə Thãgba tukɩrʋaa? Ga do afɩ i sɩ kɔɔ gba a weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔaa? Ga do afɩ i sɩ kɔɔ gba a cʋʋna nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔaa?
40007023	Liir ma so war casɩ nayɩ: Ma kɔɔ jɩ nɩnakɛ kpɩɩa', nɩ hala sa sɛ mɩ nɛrkɛ dɔnɩ sopugo cʋʋdara.
40007024	Mɛ̃ gɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ nɩɛnɛnɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔɔkɛ a yɩr da-n cʋʋ, a na hʋrɛ kũu kpɛsɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ ɔɔ cɔ boka nã thɛrɛɛra.
40007025	Dɩ thãgba nyʋɔn n daan, dɩ nyʋɔn be poo a gbʋma, dɩ jɩɛ ɩɩrɛ dɩ ga-n be cʋɔrɩle, sɩ ga jə', gɩdonɩ boka nã thɛrɛɛra wɩ thɩɩ.
40007026	Sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ nɩɛnɛnɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔɔkɛ sɩ aa-n cʋa', a na hʋrɛ kũu də̃bəəluukɛ thɛnɩ ɔɔ cɔ gbalãkothɩnna.
40007027	Dɩ thãgba nyʋɔn n daan, dɩ nyʋɔn be poo a gbʋma, dɩ jɩɛ ɩɩrɛ dɩ ga-n be cʋɔrɩle dɩɩ do gɩ təəre ji, dɩ ɔɔ jirə puurore ka.
40007028	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ thɩmɩaakɛ dɩɩ pɩ, nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ tibil jɔɔle ɔɔ dɩɩrra.
40007029	Gɩdonɩ a dɩɩr wɛr mɔ̃ a hananɩ hʋɛ, ga ho mɔ̃ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ n dɩɩr wɩna'.
40008001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ thenɩ gɔ̃gʋɔna da-n gbũ, tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ kpaaraarɛ.
40008002	Dɩ gbuul bɩɛl pʋɔraa, a gburõku ɔɔ ƴɛra, sa sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado fɩ ture fɩ punone cʋʋ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ gbuul pɩ.
40008003	Dɩ Jeju 'laa nyɔ̃ɔ a thaaraa sa sʋʋraa: Mɩ ture afɩ gbuul n pɛ. Dɩ dapaara ɔɔ gbuul pɩɩraa.
40008004	Agɩpɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ fa-n so tibillə ga, sɩ jala nɛna Thãgbaa bonɩ jidaar mɔ̃ fɩ hanɩ, a 'laanɛna phɔphʋɔl thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sonɩ, gɩ nɩna tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩ fɩ kpɛɛrɛ.
40008005	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju kɔɔ lonɩ Kapɛrnayʋm, sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl pʋɔraarɛ da-n phʋʋrʋʋ thakɛ ayɩwɔɔ:
40008006	Kɔ̃tɩn, ɩ̃ thɔ̃daar hale a gbãgbar, a phɩ̃ le cʋɔrɔ da-n 'wãga jɔɔ ka.
40008007	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Mɛrɛ, ma jaal a na kpɛsɛɛ.
40008008	Dɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩnna birsee ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ma teena dɩ fa lõ ɩ̃ cɔa', sɔ nɔ haarɩkɛrakɛ dɔrɔɔm, sɩ ɩ̃ thɔ̃daar na kpɛɛrɛ.
40008009	Gɩdonɩ mɛrɛ dakha, mɩ hananɛ ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔkɛ jɔ mɩnɩ, dɩ mɩ hananɛ dakha sɔrasɛsɔɔkɛ mɩ jɔnɩ. A mɩ so bɩɛlla: Jala, dɩ jal. A mɩ so bɩɛlla wo ayɩ: Ɩna, dɩ ɩ̃. A mɩ so ɩ̃ thɔ̃daarra: Gʋɛ gɩrɛ, dɩ cʋʋ.
40008010	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju nɩɛnɩ dɩ mɩɩna thale pɩ, nʋɔ kpagʋʋrɛ dɩ so wɩrɛraakɛ n kpaaraanɩ ayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩrarakɛ, ma kɔɔ yɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ dɩ thʋ̃ hana ha pɛrɛ dɩɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ thaka'.
40008011	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɩ so narɛ gɩrɛ, tibil jɔjʋɔ na ther wi phã paar na wi lõ paar, a na too dɩko kho paar na Abɩraham, na Ɩjakɩ, na Jakɔbɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
40008012	Sɩ wa dʋnanɛ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩɩ bɩsãsɔ jɩɛra dabirə paar na faa, ka wa bɩnɩ wa-n yɩrna nyɩma.
40008013	Agɩpɩ Jeju sor sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩnaale ayɩ: Kɔna, mɔ̃ fɩ pɛrnɩ haar ɔmɛna ga ha; dɩɩ do wa bɔraalera thɔ̃daarɩlee kho kpɛɛrɛ.
40008014	Agɩpɩ Jeju gbaar jal Pɩɛrɩ cɔ, a yɩ Pɩɛrɩ khɛrɩ nɩ dɩ phɩ̃ na tomɩ kporre,
40008015	dɩ a thaaraarɛ nyɔ̃ɔ dɩɩ do ɔɔ tomɩ kpor ɩɩraarɛ, dɩ pal ɩɩr a teguu kpakpaalɛ.
40008016	A dɩɩ dʋɔr, wɩ kɔɔ kpar kpãkpũdara jɔɔ a pɔnanaa. Dɩ a weere kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ na thɩmɩɩ bi bɩɛl, a kpɛɛna dakha khodara fɛʋ.
40008017	Dɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩ kɔɔ sonɩ dã ayɩ: “Ɔr kɔɔ wea asɩ tomɩ sɩsɔ a hɛlna asɩ khosɔ a faa.”
40008018	Mɔ̃ Jeju yɩnɩ tibil jɔ dɩ wɩ jɛ a kpalalaa, a 'laarɛ hʋɛ ɩnɩ-n ire iiro.
40008019	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar bɩɛl tɔr wɔrɔ̃ɔ a sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar, ma-n kpa farɛ paar wo paarɩkɛ fɩ-n jalnɩ.
40008020	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Ɓãɓoisɔ hananɛ awɩ ka, dɩ 'lominə hana awɩ tɛl, sɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na hana ka ma jəəni yʋa'.
40008021	Tibil bɩɛl wo kpãkpãadarara sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, ha mɩ hʋɛ ɩ̃ jal ɩ̃ dʋ ɩ̃ thɩ bo.
40008022	Sɩ Jeju birsee ayɩ: Na kpa mar sa sɛ khesɔra wa-n dʋ awɩ khisɔ.
40008023	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ lʋʋn gboroona, dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara kpaaraarɛ.
40008024	Dɩ le jɛkhu kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ɩɩr mɩɩr nɔɔra, dɩ gborõo na-n ibi nyʋɔn. Sɩ Jeju wer ha da-n daar,
40008025	dɩ kpãkpãadara tɔr pɔ a jagʋʋ sa sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, taa sɩ sɩ-n khiire.
40008026	Dɩ bule wi ayɩ: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ maar fʋ nɩ, nɛrɛɛkɛ kanɩ hana ha pɛrɛ gbe? Le a ɩɩr a mana jɩɛ na mɩɩr nɔɔ, dɩ thɩ̃ɛ na-n tutugo bã.
40008027	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ tɩbɩlaale dɩ wa-n bule ayɩ: Anyee tibil ca ha ʋrɛ ya fɛ, dɩ jɩɛrakɛ na mɩɩr nɔɔ na-n nɩɩ nũu?
40008028	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju iirni gɩ̃ iiro Gadarɛ̃daraa dʋɔ na pɩ, kona yenyɔɔkɛ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbii ther khi dʋ paar dɩ wa-n caanʋʋ. Wɩ-n kʋrɛ maar ka, dɩ tibil na-n 'la dɩ kana hʋɛɛla'.
40008029	Dɩ wɩ mar dɩ wa-n hulẽ ayɩ: Anye sɩ ha kha na fɛr, Thãgbaa Bikuun? Fɩ ɩnɛ kɛ fɩ hʋɔl sar, sɩ bɔɔ na dã na paa ya?
40008030	Sɩ dabulo sɩthɔ jɔɔ wɛ a kɔɔ hale ƴɔɔ dɩ wa-n khʋʋl.
40008031	Dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiirə na-n phʋʋr Jeju thakɛ ayɩ: Ado fɩ wee sɩ, thɔna sɩ sɩ lõ sɩthɔsɔraale.
40008032	Dɩ a so warɛ: Nɩ jala. Dɩ wɩ thɩɩr a jal a lõ sɩthɔsɔraale bɩnɔ, a tinə wi fɛʋ dɩ wɩ ca birbirbir na gɔ̃gɔ̃ horʋ, a jiir mɩɩr nɔɔra, a khiir le nyʋɔnɔ.
40008033	Dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ n khɛ wɩnɩ, wɩ kɔɔ car kɔ̃, a mɩɩ dɩɩra thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na gɩrɛ kɔɔ dananɩ kuunnaakɛ kɔɔ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ.
40008034	Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩɩra ther jal Jejuu pa; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ, wɩ phʋʋrʋʋrɛ ayɩ a thɛ nɩ dɩɩra.
40009001	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ lʋʋn gboroona a iir lanyʋɔn, sa gba kɔ̃ ɔɔ dʋɔ.
40009002	Dɩ hɩnɛ, wɩ kɔɔ gbaar gbãgbarʋʋkɛ n phɩnanɩ phɩ̃ paar a pɔnanaa. Dɩ mɔ̃ Jeju yɩnɩ awɩ ha pɛ, a sor gbãgbarʋra: Pɩɛr 'lar ɩ̃ bɩsã, afɩ sopugo hɛl farɛ.
40009003	Dɩ wɩ̃ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ n sor na awɩ bɩ̃ ayɩ: Thãgbaa i kuunikɛ n kʋɛ.
40009004	Dɩ mɔ̃ Jeju jɩnɩ awɩ kpɩɛr, a bule wer ayɩ: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nɩ hana kpɩɛr puu thakɛ anɩ bɩnɔ?
40009005	Gɩmɔ̃ yɔɔnɛ sorra: Afɩ sopugo hɛl farɛ gɩ yaa, agɩbo ɩrɛ jala gɩ?
40009006	Sɩ mɔ̃ na fʋnɩ sɩ na jɩ, dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun hananɛ hʋɛ thɩɩra dɩ ɩ̃ faana sopugo, sa bir so gbãgbarʋra: Ɩrɛ, gba afɩ phɩ̃ pa na kɔna.
40009007	Dɩ a ɩɩrɛ da-n kɔ̃ ɔɔ cɔ.
40009008	Mɔ̃ tibil jɔɔle yɩnɩ gele, maar fʋlɛ wɛr dɩ wa-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaakɛ hananɩ tɩbɩla ga puno caale.
40009009	Dɩ Jeju tɔr na jal gbe, a yɩ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Matiə dɩ too war gba paar da-n tee war, dɩ sʋʋraa: Na kpa mar. Dɩ Matiə ɩɩr da-n kpaaraa.
40009010	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ har dɩko kho paar cʋɔrɔ, dɩ war gbadara jɔɔ na sopugodara kɔɔ toonanɛ kha Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadarasɔ.
40009011	Mɔ̃ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara yɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ thale, wɩ sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ anɩ dɩɩrdaar na-n kho dɩkɔ na war gbadara na sopugodarasɔ?
40009012	Dɩ mɔ̃ Jeju nɩɛnɩ gele, a so warɛ: Ga do tɩɩ khena n kɔɔ ƴaalɛ dɔtɔrɔa', sɩ wɩrɛ gɩ-n khonɩ gɩ.
40009013	Nɩ jala na dɩrɛ a jɛ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛɛ kɩr, kɛ sɔnɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩwɔɔ: “Bɔ donanɛ mɛr Thãgba n ƴaal, ga do bonɩ jir ga.” Gɩdonɩ ga do fɩl sardara mɩ ɩ̃ ɩ̃ ƴaala', sɩ sopugodara wɛ.
40009014	Le Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ kpãkpãadarasɔ pɔ Jejura a bulee: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ se wer na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na-n li nʋɔ, sɩ afɩ kpãkpãadarasɔ wer na-n li nʋɔa'.
40009015	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ wenɩ herra na punone wa-n bɩ bɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ kha na khɛr he ya? Sɩ wiresɔ na hale wa hɛl warnɩ khɛr he. Le wa li nʋɔ dɩphã.
40009016	Tibil na gba kẽkẽ phaa na kur na bɛbɩna kẽkẽ tɩ̃a', gɩdonɩ daphaale na-n haalɛ datɩ̃ɩ, gɩ do gɩ ka ɓəəre dɩphã waa a ka puuro ka.
40009017	Wa-n gba dakha thʋʋrɩkɛ dɔnɩ daphaa a pɛ bʋla tɩɩna ga. A wɩ cʋʋ mɛ̃, bʋlaa na wɩɛlɛ dɩ thʋʋr na deer, gɩ do bʋlaale kʋɛrɛ mɛ̃. Sɩ wɩ-n pɛr thʋ phaa bʋla phaara oti dɩɩ gbɛbɩ too.
40009018	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ hanɩ da-n mɩɩ wɩ ga thɩmɩɩsɔɔkɛ, kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl pɔr dã a gburõkuraa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa so: Ɩ̃ bikhɛr khire ga pʋɔr pa', sɩ ɩna a dɛɛnaa nyɛ̃ɛ a na bɩre na hana yɩre.
40009019	Dɩ Jeju ɩɩrɛ da-n kpaaraa nakha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara.
40009020	Dɩ hɩnɛ khɛ bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hale a hana tɩ̃ɩ a cʋʋna yɛna yuɔr yenyɔ, dɩ a tɔr pɔ Jejura khiro a thaaraaa kẽkẽ nʋɔra.
40009021	Gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ sor le na ɔɔ bɩ̃ ayɩ: A mɩ punonakɛ a thar ɔɔ kẽkẽ haraakɛrakɛ sɩ ma kpɛɛrɛ.
40009022	Dɩ mɔ̃ Jeju kɩɩlnɩ a yɩɩ a sʋʋraarɛ: Pɩɛr 'lar ɩ̃ bikhɛr, afɩ ha pɛ kpɛɛnɛ fɩ; dɩ dapaara khɛrɩlee kho kpɛɛ.
40009023	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju danɩ kɔ̃tɩnɩ cɔ, a yɩrɛ bel ʋ̃dara na tɩbɩla jɔɔ dɩ wa-n khɔ̃, dɩ a so warɛ:
40009024	Nɩ tɔ birə gɩdonɩ khebirrə na khə', sɩ a-n daarɛ; sɩ wɩ-n maanʋʋnɛ.
40009025	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a tini tibil jɔɔle dɩ wɩ thɩɩr, a lʋʋn a fʋ khebirrə nyɔ̃ɔ dɩ pal ɩɩr.
40009026	Dɩ ga tutugo kɔɔ kpaarɛ paar fɛʋ ga bənəəle.
40009027	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju thenɩ le da-n jal, yara yenyɔ n kpaaraarɛ dɩ wa-n hulẽ ayɩ: Jɛ sɩ bʋɔrarakɛ ya, Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun.
40009028	Dɩ mɔ̃ a lonɩ cʋɔrɔ na pɩ, yaraale pɔr wɔrɔ̃ɔ dɩ bule wi: Nɩ pɛrɛ haar ma punone gelela a na cʋʋ ya? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Ɔɔ, Kɔ̃tɩn.
40009029	Dɩ le a tha war yinəna sa so: Mɔ̃ anɩ ha pɛ hanɩ, ɔmɛna ga ha.
40009030	Dɩ awɩ yi khɛrrɛ. Sɩ Jeju jɩɛ kpãkpãa war thakɛ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ: Nɩ jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, na-n do tibil n jɩ thɩ̃ɛɛka';
40009031	sɩ mɔ̃ wa thenɩ, dapaara wɩ mar ɔɔda a be dɩ wa-n wɩɛl ga bənəəle koo.
40009032	Mɔ̃kɛ wa thenɩ le, wɩ kpar kuunikɛ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbu nɔ madaar a pɔnanaa.
40009033	Dɩ a weeraarɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuule sɩ dɩ nɔ madaarɩle na-n mɩɩ thɩmɩa dɩphã. Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ tibil jɔɔle dɩ wa-n so: Sa kɔɔ yɩ thɩ̃ɛ thakɛ Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩra kpɩɩraka'.
40009034	Sɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ wer na-n so ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ n hanaa fãga dɩ weena kɔ̃tɛɛbii.
40009035	Dɩ Jeju n kɔɔ kpaarɛ dɩ kɔ̃tɩnasɔra fɛʋ na dɩ biisɔra, da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ, da-n mɩɩna tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ ƴũ fãgadaar doda, da-n kpɛɛna khoosɔ dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ na tãdarasɔ dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ.
40009036	Sɩ mɔ̃ a yɩnɩ tibil jɔɔle, bʋɔ fʋʋrɛ gɩdonɩ wɩ thʋnɛ vɔɔ dɩɩ ka war, dɩ wa-n puno bã a ho banaakɛ na hananɩ khekha'.
40009037	Dɩ le a so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Jɔ jɔrɛ, sɩ jʋ kha na kpɛra'.
40009038	Gɛr gɩ na-n bɩɛlnɛ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn jʋ kharra a thɔna thɔ̃dara wa-n kha jɔ.
40010001	Agɩpɩ dɩ Jeju we ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ a ha wɩ punone dɩ wa-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔlasɔ, wa-n kpɛɛna khoosɔ dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ na tãdarasɔ dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ.
40010002	Thɔ̃thɔna yʋɔr yenyɔɔ isɔra ha gɩrɛ: Gacadaar Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pɩɛr na ɔɔ õkuun Ãdire, Jakɩ Jebedee bikuun na Jã ɔɔ õkuun,
40010003	Filipi na Bartelemɩ, Tomasɩ na Matiəəkɛ dɔnɩ war gbadaar, Jakɩ Alfee bikuun, na Tade,
40010004	Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ dʋɔnnɩ gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ tibil, na Judasɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ dɩɩra, kɛ lirenanɩ Jeju.
40010005	Wɛr dɔ yʋɔr yenyɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ thɔnɩ a so war thakɛ ayɩ: Na-n jal thɩldaraa pa ga, na-n lõ Samarɩdarasɔɔ dɩsɔra ga.
40010006	Sɩ nɩ ka na jala Ɩjɩrayɛl ca wɩrɛra bureni a ho banaa.
40010007	Sɩ mɔ̃ nɩ-n jalnɩ na-n mɩa ayɛ, bɔɔ n daan dɩ ƴũ Fãgadaar na-n gba fãga.
40010008	Na-n kpɛɛnɛ khodarasɔ dakha, na-n ɩrɛ khesɔ khirera, na-n cʋɛ gbulosɔɔ gbuul ga-n pɩ, na-n wea kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ na faa. Khaar nɩ 'lɛ, na-n 'laanɛ khaar.
40010009	Na-n gba dɛ a fʋrɔa', na-n gba war dɩ war yɩra gɩ a to lokaara';
40010010	na-n fʋrɔ kpakpaar lokaara', na-n gba kẽkena yenyɔa', na-n to nɛfaa ga, na-n fʋrɔ gbʋʋla', gɩdonɩ thɔ̃daar teenanɛ haanɛ.
40010011	Dɩ dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ dɔɔraakɛ na lonɩ, a dɩ buurə gɩ, nɩ bulene ado tibil hale kɛ teananɩ a na tee nɩ. Nɩ tɔɔ le ntɛɛ pa phaphapha gɩ dana wireekɛ na thenɩ le.
40010012	Sɩ ado na lõ cɔ dɔɔra, nɩ kɔɔ fʋɔrɛɛ.
40010013	Ado cɔ dɔɔ teere kha, anɩ ha ie n ɓananaa, sɩ ado cɔ dɔɔ na tee kha ga, anɩ ha ie n birə nar.
40010014	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wa-n tee nɩna', dɩ ga do wɩ-n pɛ anɩ thɩmɩɩ nũu dakha ga, nɩ thɛ cɔ dɔɔrara agɩbo dɩ dɔɔrara, sa kpɛɛnɛ thɩlãkobe anɩ nɛra.
40010015	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, Sɔdɔmdara na Gɔmɔɔrdaraa kɩɩlɩkɛ wa 'lɛnɩ na khɩɩr mɔ̃ dɩɩlee kɩɩl na khɩɩrna'.
40010016	Sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, banaa nɩ ho dɩ ɩ̃ thɔ̃ kpesɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn; gɛr gɩ nɩ kpɛsɛnɛ sii kha sa hana hɛlɛlɛ a hɔ puusɩ̃ɛ.
40010017	Sɩ na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ tɩbɩlala, gɩdonɩ wa fʋlɛ nɛr na jalna kɩɩl paar, wa ciil ner na khasa Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra.
40010018	Mɛr na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ̃ wa fʋlɛ nɩ na jalna gobanɛrsɔ na fãgadarasɔɔ ƴɛra, gɩ mɩɩ wɩ anɩ ha pɛda na ca kpala dakha.
40010019	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wa liirna nɩnɩ, na-n dɛ mɔ̃kɛ na mɩɩnɩ, agɩbo gɩrɛɛkɛ na sona'. Gɩrɛ na sonɩ na ɩ̃ narɛ ga bɔraalera.
40010020	Gɩdonɩ ga do nɛr na mɩa ga, sɩ anɩ Thɩɩ Thu gɩɩkɛ na mɩanɩ le anɩ bɩnɔ na ha nɩ.
40010021	õkuun na liirnanɛ ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔ dɩ wa kʋ; ɔmɛ̃ thɩrɛ na cʋʋ na ɔɔ bɩsã. Bɩsana dakha na ɩɩrɛ na tɛna thɛ na nɛ na cʋʋ dɩ wa kʋʋr wɩ.
40010022	Tɩbɩla fɛʋ na laar nɛr, gɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ, sɩ ʋrɛ na yɩranɩ na dana khu paar, ɔr na 'lɛ taarɛ.
40010023	A wɩ kpoo nar dɩ bɩɛlla, nɩ fuo ca ka dɩ kpɩɩra. Sɩ sobɔr mɩ so nar, na kpaar Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩ fɛʋ na pɩ sɩɩ do mɛr tibili Bikuun bire ɩ̃a'.
40010024	Kpãkpãadaar na hale a na kɔ̃tɩ̃ na jɔ ʋrɛ n dɩrɛɛna', dɩ thɔ̃daar wo na hale a na kɔ̃tɩ̃ na jɔ ɔɔ kɔ̃tã'.
40010025	Gɩ daan dɩ wa hɩɩn kpãkpãadaar mɔ̃ wɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ ʋrɛ n dɩrɛɛnɩ, wɩ hɩɩn thɔ̃daar dakha mɔ̃ wɩ hɩɩnnɩ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃. Ado wɩ we cɔdaar kuun Bɛljɛbul, dɩ mɔ̃ wa ka na we dɩphã ɔɔ cɔdara?
40010026	Gɛr gɩ na-n ma wɩ kpɩɩa', gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ker sɩɩ do ga yɩraa ga, dɩ thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ha gbul sɩɩ do wa jɩ gaaga.
40010027	Gɩrɛ mɩ khe narnɩ pa birə paar, nɩ sɔ gɩ dahɩrɛra tɩbɩla n nɩɛ. Gɩrɛ nɩ nɩɛnɩ bʋ̃bʋʋnɛna, nɩ hulene gi nãsʋrɔ.
40010028	Na-n ma wɩrɛ n kɔnɩ tomɩr, sɩ wa-n puno thue dɩ wɩ kʋaa ga, sɩ nɩ ka na ma ʋrɛ hananɩ punone a na cʋʋ dɩ anɩ thu na anɩ tomɩ na kʋɛ bu paar dɔɔra.
40010029	Wa-n dolõ 'lominə yenyɔ war be yenyɔaa? Sɩrakɛ bɩɛl na puno na ji thʋnɔ, sɩ agado anɩ Thɩ tuonaa ga.
40010030	Anɩ thɛthɛɛ yʋsũsɔrakɛ Thãgba ther ger fɛʋ.
40010031	Gɛr gɩ na-n do maar na-n fʋ na', anɩ the nɔ khɩɩrɛ a jɔ 'lomĩ jɔjɔjʋɔ.
40010032	Gɛr gɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na tuon mini tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra, mɛrɛ dakha ma tuure ɩ̃ Thɩraakɛ hanɩle ƴũu ƴɛra.
40010033	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ bɔ mɩnɩ tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra, mɛrɛ dakha ma bor ntɛɛle ɩ̃ Thɩraakɛ hanɩle ƴũu ƴɛra dakha.
40010034	Na-n kpɩɛr ha ɩɩ mɩ ɩna ɩ̃ 'laa thɩɩra ga. Ma ɩ̃ ɩ̃ 'laa ha ɩa', sɩ bajɩna gɩ.
40010035	Gɩdonɩ mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ pɛr leere bikuunna na ɔɔ thɩ, bikhɩɛnna na ɔɔ nɩ, khɛrra na ɔɔ koo nɩ dakha,
40010036	dɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ tibili cɔdara na fien na do ɔɔ lãlaardara.
40010037	Ʋrɛ n naannɩ ɔɔ thɩ, a ɔɔ nɩ gɩ, a jɔ mɩ aa teena ma'; dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n naannɩ ɔɔ bikuun, a ɔɔ bikhɛr gɩ, a jɔ mɩ aa teena ma'.
40010038	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n gbaannɩ ɔɔ kʋkʋ thɩr dɩ heen da-n kpana mara', aa teena ma'.
40010039	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n tɛbanɩ ɔɔ yi, ga ka na buurəəre, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛɛ yi na kanɩ na bu mɛrɛra, ɔr na lɛ waa gel.
40010040	Ʋrɛ tea nɩnɩ, mɛr a tee, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ tea mɩnɩ, ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ a tee dakha.
40010041	Ʋrɛ teanɩ Thãgbaa bobon Thãgbaa bobon teguu, a na 'lɛr khor Thãgbaa bobonɩ kha; dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ teanɩ tɩɩ sarʋ tɩɩ sar teguu, a na 'lɛr khor tɩɩ sarʋʋ kha.
40010042	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na cɛnɩ yɔ ie haarɩkɛrakɛ na ha ɩ̃ kpãkpãadaar pɩɛrʋʋkɛ, gɩdonɩ mɛrra a-n kpa dɩɩ do gɛr dɔ nɔɔ, sobɔr mɩ so nar, ntɛ na 'lee ɔɔ khoa'.
40011001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ pɩ, a ther le a jal da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla da-n mɩɩna wɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ awɩ dɩsɔra.
40011002	Jãakɛ wɩ kɔɔ fʋnɩ a to khaɩra, a nɩɛrɛ thɔmaakɛ Kirisiti n cʋʋnɩ, dɩ a thʋɔn ɔɔ kpãkpãadara wɩ jala bulenee ayɛwɔɔ:
40011003	Fɛr dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛra na ɩnanɩ yaa, agɩbo dɔ sa-n pɩɛr tɩɩ kpɩɩ?
40011004	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Nɩ kɛra birə a sɔ Jana gɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ-n nɩɛnɩ na gɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ:
40011005	Yarasɔ n yɩrɛ, nɛ kʋɛdarasɔ n sar bɔɔbɔɔ, gbulosɔɔ gbuul pɩrɛ, dɩ nʋrasɔ khɛrrɛ, dɩ khesɔ n ɩɩrɛ dɩ wɩ the khirera, dɩ bɔdara nɩɛrɛ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ.
40011006	Sɩ gɩ da ʋrɛraakɛ ma doronɩ nɛ baradaa ga.
40011007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ kɔnɩ na pɩ, Jeju mar da-n mɩɩ tibil jɔɔle Jãadara aa: Anye nɩ kɔɔ ka jal bəənnə a hɩɩn? Poo balãsɩɩkɛ jɩɛ n khəəfəni gɩ ya?
40011008	Dɩ anye nɩ kɔɔ jal yɩ? Kuunikɛ n tɔnɩ kẽkẽ ɓʋ̃ɔ gɩ ya? Nɩ hɩnɛ wo wɩrɛɛkɛ n tɔnɩ kẽkẽ ɓɔna fãgadaraa cɔ wɩ-n ha.
40011009	Dɩ anye nɩ kɔɔ jal yɩ? Thãgbaa bobon gɩ ya? Mɩ so narɛ, sobɔr gɩ, bɩɛlɩkɛ jɔnɩ Thãgbaa bobon gɩ.
40011010	Jãada dɔ gɩrɛ kheranɩ kɩɛr Thãgbaa sɛbɛraakɛ ayɩ: “Hɩnɛ, mɛr Thãgba thɔna ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃, dɩ na kʋʋl fɩ ƴɩɛ, a gbɛbɩrɩ fɩ hʋɛ afɩ ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ.”
40011011	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ khɛra n kɔnɩɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, bɩɛl na hale a ɩɩr a kɔ̃tɩ̃ a jɔ Jã Batɩsɩtɩ kpɩɩraka'. Sɩ ʋrɛ kanɩ do dabuu fɩɩʋ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra, a kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ Jã.
40011012	A fʋna Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ bɔɔ a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ, wɩ-n pɛrɛ fãga dɩ wa-n lõ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra, dɩ wɩrɛ n pɩɛrnɩ fãga, wɛr hɩna.
40011013	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa bobonasɔ fɛʋ na jɔfʋ, gɩ kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ Thãgbaa so a dana Jãa bɔɔ.
40011014	Dɩ ado nɩ ƴaalɛ nɩ tu gi, ɔr dɔ Elɩra teananɩ a ɩna.
40011015	Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
40011016	Ana ma cʋna nĩdaraakɛ dɩphã ya fɛ? Wɩ hʋrɛ bɩsanasɔɔkɛ n tɔɔnɩ ƴatɔɔ, dɩ wa-n we awɩ 'walãkhasɔ dɩ wa-n so:
40011017	Sɩ kɔɔ ʋnɛ bɩɩl nɛrɛra, sɩ na kɔɔ sa ga, sɩ kɔɔ khɩɩrɛ nɛrɛra, sɩ na kɔɔ ba'.
40011018	Gɩdonɩ Jã kɔɔ ɩnɛ, aa-n kɔɔ kho dɩkora', aa-n kɔɔ yɔ thɩ̃a', dɩ wɩ jɩɩl sa yɩ: Kɔ̃tɛɛbuu hanaanɛ.
40011019	Dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ɩ̃ wo, a thɩ̃ɛ mɩ-n kho, a thɩ̃ɛ mɩ-n yɔ, dɩ wɩ jɩɩl wo sa yɩ: Hɩnɛ, kũu kɛ̃kɛbɩ gɩ, a dona ta yɔn, war gbadara na sopugodaraa kuun gɩ. Sɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa kpɛsɛ n cʋʋnɩ n nɩnanɛ dɩ sobɔr har kpɛsɛrɛɛlee pa.
40011020	Le Jeju ma da-n phaan dɩɩsɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ cʋʋrɔnɩ ɔɔ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃sɔ jɔɔ, gɩdonɩ ha debire na kɔɔ hala', ayɩ:
40011021	Ga puu farɛ Korajɛ̃ dɩɩ, ga puu farɛ Bɛcaɩda dɩɩ, gɩdonɩ ado nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ cʋɛnɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ mɛ̃ Tɩɩr na Sɩdɔ̃ dɩɩra, wa kɔɔ mãa debire haar kɛkɛkɛ, sɩ na to bɔrɔ na bʋlna thoo.
40011022	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so nar: Wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, Tɩɩrdara na Sɩdɔ̃daraa kɩɩlɩkɛ wa 'lɛnɩ na khɩɩr mɔ̃ anɩ kɩɩl na khɩɩrna'.
40011023	Sɩ fɛrɛ Kapɛrnayʋm dɩɩ, Thãgba na khəi fer na jʋʋnna ƴũ ya? Ǝ̃'ə̃, Thãgba na gbumo fer dɩ fa thʋ khĩdi dɩɩ. Gɩdonɩ ado nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ afɩ pa Sɔdɔm gɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ, ga dor a na kɔɔ hale na dana nĩ.
40011024	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so nar: Wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, Sɔdɔmdaraa kɩɩlɩkɛ wa 'lɛnɩ na khɩɩr mɔ̃ anɩ kɩɩl na khɩɩrna'.
40011025	Ga bɔɔlera Jeju gba thɩmɩa da-n mɩɩ ayɩ: Thɩrɛ, mɩ-n fʋɔr fɛr, fɛrkɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩra, gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ kɔɔ kernɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛra kpɛsɛdarara na thɩ̃ jɩnana, sa gba gɩ a nɩna bɩsã bii.
40011026	Ɔɔ Thɩrɛ, fɛr gɩ kɔɔ da haar dɩ fɩ cʋʋ mɛ̃.
40011027	Ɩ̃ Thɩ gbaar thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ a dʋ mɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ, sɩ tibil na jɩ Bikuun saagado Thɩrɛ gaaga, dɩ tibil na jɩ Thɩrɛ dakha saagado Bikuun gaaga, saagado wo Bikuunna ɔr ƴaalɛ a nɩrɔ n taa ga.
40011028	Nɩ ɩna mɛrɛra, nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n vɔɔnɩ kɛ n heenenɩ dakha heendaakɛ dɩbarɔnɩ, dɩ ma ha nɛr hɩɩrɛ.
40011029	Nɩ tɔ kpeleleekɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃da, dɩ nɩ to ɩ̃ dɩɩrsɔ, gɩdonɩ hɛlɛlɛ fɩldaar na ha jodaar ha mɩ, dɩ na 'lɛr hɩɩrɛ anɩ hara.
40011030	Gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ kpeleekɛ ma to nɩnɩ, gɩ habarɛ; dɩ ɩ̃ heendaakɛ ma heen nɩnɩ, ga dɩbɩrɔa'.
40012001	Ga bɔɔlera Jeju n kɔɔ ka a lõ jʋ lɩɛra hɩɩr wire. Dɩ kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋrɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, dɩ wɩ mar a 'laa kha jɔ dɩ wa-n kho.
40012002	Dɩ mɔ̃ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ yɩ gɩnɩ, wɩ sʋʋraarɛ ayɩ: Hɩnɛ, afɩ kpãkpãadara n cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ yɩnɩ gɩ-n sãsɩrɛ hɩɩr wire.
40012003	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Na kɔɔ yɩɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra gɩrɛɛkɛ Davɩdɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋʋnɩ ɔr na wɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ kha gaa?
40012004	Mee a kɔɔ lʋʋn Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ a gba buruukɛ wɩ-n hanɩ Thãgba dɩ wɩ kho, sɩrakɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ na tɩbɩlaale a kɔɔ hananɩ kha na kɔɔ hana hʋɛ a na kho ga, Thãgbaa gbõdara dɩbaraada gɩ.
40012005	Dɩ na ba yɩ gɩ jɔfʋ sɛbɛra wo, mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa gbõdara n cʋʋnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ gɩrɛ dɩ wa-n kʋɛ hɩɩr wire, sɩ wa-n 'lɛ soraa gaa?
40012006	Dɩ mɩ ka so narɛ ʋkhaakɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔr hakɛ.
40012007	Ado nɩ kɔɔ jɩrɛ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛɛ kɩr, kɛ sɔnɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Bɔ donanɛ mɛr Thãgba n ƴaal, ga do bonɩ jir ga” na kɔɔ heen wɩrɛkɛ na hananɩ dɩa sora'.
40012008	Gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun dʋɔn Kɔ̃tɩn hɩɩr wirerarakɛ.
40012009	Sɩ Jeju ther le a gba jal lõ awɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra.
40012010	Dɩ le a yɩ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ nyɔ̃ɔ khini. Sɩ gɩdonɩ wɩ-n ƴaalɛ hʋɛ wɩ pɛr Jeju sor, wɩ buleele ayɩ: Hɩɩr wire teenanɛ kho kpɛɛrɛ ya?
40012011	Dɩ a birse wer: Ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil nɛrɛra, ado a hana bana bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ dɩ ji kõkorro hɩɩr wire, a na halʋʋ na təə?
40012012	Dɩ tibil na khɩɩr the nʋɔ a jɔ banaa fiiəə? Dɩ gɛr gɩ hɩɩr wire teena bɔ cʋʋrɛ.
40012013	Dɩ le a so kuunnaale ayɩ: 'Laanɛ afɩ nyɔ̃, dɩ 'laa dɩɩ do gɩ kpɛɛrɛ a ha mɔ̃ ʋ̃ nyɔ̃ hanɩ.
40012014	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ ther dɩ wa-n gʋʋr kha mɔ̃ wa fʋnɩ sɩ na kʋ Jeju.
40012015	Dɩ Jeju nɩɛrɛ gele a faa paarɩle sa the. Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ kpaaraarɛ, dɩ a kpɛɛrɛ khodara fɛʋ;
40012016	sɩ a-n kpãkpãa warɛ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ, wa-n so ntɛ ɩnɩ dona'.
40012017	Gɩ do mɛ̃ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ Ejaɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ dã oti:
40012018	“Hɩnɛ, ɔr dʋɔn thɔ̃daarɩkɛ mɛr Thãgba phiirni, ʋrɛ mɩ-n nanɩ gɩ, a lõ mer haar kpɛ. Ma pɩɛraarɛ ɩ̃ Thu, dɩ a na mɩɩrɛ fɩl sarʋ tibil caar fɛʋra.
40012019	A na bana thɩ̃ banaa ga, a na hulə̃', dɩ tibil bɩɛl na nɩ ɔɔ nɔ dɩ bɩnɔ dakha ga.
40012020	A na kha jʋmũukɛ hanɩ kpɛlɛ kpɛlɛ na fa ga. A na khiir dakha lãphã pɔ̃ɔkɛ n dɔnɩnakɛ isi haara', phaphapha a cʋʋ fɩl sarʋ gɩ kəə.
40012021	Dɩ ɔr tibil caar fɛʋ na-n pɛ nũu.”
40012022	Le wɩ kpa kuunikɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuu cʋʋnɩ dɩ do nɔ madaar a yaarna a pɔna Jejura, dɩ wee kɔ̃tɛɛbuu a faa, dɩ nɔ madaarɩle mɩɩrɛ nʋɔ da-n yɩna dɩphã.
40012023	Dɩ nʋɔ kpaarɛ tibil jɔɔle fɛʋ dɩ wa-n so: Dɩ ɔr ba dɔ Davɩdɩɩ Bikuunna yaa?
40012024	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara nɩɛnɩ gele, wɩ sor ayɩ: Kuunikɛ na-n wee kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ saagado na Bɛljɛbulikɛ dɔnɩ yʋʋ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔraa fãga gaaga.
40012025	Mɔ̃ Jeju jɩnɩ awɩ kpɩɛr, a so warɛ: Fãgadaar dɩ wo fãgadaar dɩɩkɛ n tɩnɛnɛnɩ a bir da-n kena dɩbara, a na wɩɛlɛ; dɩ dɩɩ wo dɩɩkɛ agɩbo, cʋɔr wo cʋɔrɩkɛ tɩnɛnɛnɩ a bir da-n kena dɩbara, ga puno na jɩɩla'.
40012026	Dɩ ado Satã na wee Satã, a tɩnɛ a bir da-n kena dɩbara, mɔ̃ ɔɔ fãgadaar dɩ na fʋ sɩ na jɩɩl?
40012027	Dɩ ado mɛrɛ Bɛljɛbuli fãga mɩ-n gba dɩ ma-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ, sɩ anɩ bɩsãsɔ amɛɛ i wɩ-n gba dɩ wa-n weena wɩ? Dɩ gɛr gɩ anɩ thɛthɛɛ bɩsãsɔra na dʋɔn anɩ so kɩɩldara.
40012028	Dɩ ado mɛrɛ, Thãgbaa Thu mɩ-n gba dɩ ma-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ, ga dor Thãgbaa fãgadaar do dã nɛr mɛ̃ dɩphã.
40012029	Mɔ̃ tibil na fʋ sɩ na lõ na fãga kũu khɩɩ cɔ na taaraa thɩ̃ɛsɔ, saagado kũu khɩɩlera a kɔɔ fʋ ɓo a lə? Ado a punoo ɓo dɩphã, gɛr a na taaraa thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ cʋɔrɔ.
40012030	Ʋrɛ na-n hanɩ kha na mɛrɛa', ɩ̃da a-n bo, dɩ wo ʋrɛ na-n bulo mini sɩ kpa ga, ɔr n bɩ̃bɩlanɛ gɩ.
40012031	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so nar ayɩwɔɔ: Thãgba na faarɛ sopugo caar dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ na i kʋɛ caar dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋʋkɛ tɩbɩla n cʋʋnɩ a na-n ha wɩ, sɩ ʋrɛ na kʋɛanɩ Thu Phuu i, Thãgba na faa ga sopugo caale kpɩɩraka'.
40012032	Dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na mɩanɩ thɩmɩɩ puu na pɛ mɛr tibili Bikuunna, Thãgba na faarɛ ga sopugo caale na haa, sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na mɩanɩ thɩmɩɩ puu na pɛ Thu Phuurə, Thãgba na faa ga sopugo caale kpɩɩrakɛ na haa, dɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ gɩ, dɩ bɔɔraakɛ na ɩnanɩ ga.
40012033	A nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ thɩrʋ bɔrɛ, oti ɔɔ bi n bɔr. A nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ thɩrʋ puurore, oti ɔɔ bi n puuro. Gɩdonɩ be wɩ-n jɩna thɩrʋ.
40012034	Nɛr sikori bisɔ, mɔ̃ ner na kɔɔ punona na mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ bʋɔ, puu ca ʋrɛ nɩ thʋnɩ puuro? Gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ henɩ bɩnɔ, gɛr nʋɔ n mɩɩ.
40012035	Tɩɩ bʋɔ n tire dabʋɔ ɔɔ thɩ̃ bɔra. Dɩ tɩɩ puu n tire dapuu ɔɔ thɩ̃ puurə.
40012036	Mɩ so narɛ, wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, thɩmɩɩ mɔlɔsɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ wa ther ger fɛʋ na ha wɩ.
40012037	Gɩdonɩ afɩ thɩmɩɩ na cʋɛ sor dɩ ga hɛl far, dɩ afɩ thɩmɩɩ na cʋɛ wo dɩ sor na heen fɩ.
40012038	Le ɩkhaa jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ hana thɩmɩɩr a so Jejura ayɩwɔɔ: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ-n ƴaalɛ fɩ cʋɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ bɩɛl sɩ yɩ gɩ.
40012039	Dɩ birse wi: Nĩdaraakɛ puuroni thakɛ, kɛ faanɩ awɩ Thãgba, n ƴaalɛlakɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ, sɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kpɩɩ na bir na yɩ saagado Jonasɩ Thãgbaa bobonɩda gaaga.
40012040	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ Jonasɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ wire yẽther na dɩtɩnɛ yẽther thʋ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ, ɔmɛ̃ mɛr tibili Bikuun na cʋʋ wire yẽther na dɩtɩnɛ yẽther thɩɩkɛɛ bɩnɔ.
40012041	Wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, Nɩnɩvɩdara na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera nakha nĩdaraakɛ, dɩ wɛr na heene wɩ sor, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ debire haar ɔbɔɔkɛ Jonasɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ. Sɩ nɩ ka hɩnɛ ʋkhaakɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ Jonasɩ hakɛ.
40012042	Wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, khɛr fãgadaarɩkɛ kɔɔ hanɩ wi phã paar nyɔ̃bɩlana na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera nakha nĩdaraakɛ, dɩ ɔr na heene wɩ sor. Gɩdonɩ ɔr, thɩ khu paar a kɔɔ the a pɔ a pɛ Salomɔ̃ɔ kpɛsɛ nũu. Sɩ nɩ ka hɩnɛ ʋkhaakɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ Salomɔ̃ hakɛ.
40012043	Ɔbɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl n thenɩ tibillə, a-n jaal da-n kpaar bə̃ kparaara, da-n ƴaal kãkɛ a na toonɩ na hɩɩr, sɩ aa-n yɩ gɩ kpɩɩa'.
40012044	Agɩpɩ a-n sor dɩ yɩ: Ma kɛrrɛ na bir ɩ̃ cɔ kãkɛ mɩ kɔɔ thenɩ. Ado a pɔ dã a yɩ cʋɔrɩle dɩɩ do dakhɩɩ, dɩ wɩ kpabɩ sa gbɛbɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ bɔɔbɔɔ,
40012045	le a-n jal dɩphã mɛ̃ dɩ kpa kɔ̃tɛɛbi kpɩɩsɔ wo makonyɔɔkɛ n hʋɔlɛnɩ dɩ wɩ jʋɔ, dɩ wɩ pɔ a lõ a too le. Dɩ mɔ̃ ga hanɩ tibilləəle pɩpɩɩ paar, ga ka na puurore na jɔ caca fʋ paar. Mɛ̃ ga ha gɩrɛ na nĩda puu ca ƴɩrɛ.
40012046	Mɔ̃ Jeju hanɩ da-n mɩɩna tibil jɔɔle, ɔɔ nɩ na ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔsɔ pɔr a jɩɩl phiilo, dɩ wa-n ƴaal wɩ mɩɩnaa.
40012047	Dɩ ʋkha sʋʋraa: Hɩnɛ, afɩ nɩ na afɩ õkũu bɩnɔsɔ hale phiilo a ƴaal wɩ mɩɩna fɩ.
40012048	Dɩ Jeju birsee ayɩ: Amɛ n dʋɔn ɩ̃ nɩ, na ɩ̃ õkona, na ɩ̃ õkhɛrsɔ?
40012049	Agɩpɩ dɩ 'laa nyɔ̃ɔ ɔɔ kpãkpãadarasɔra sa so: Nɩ yɛ kɛ ɩ̃ nɩ na ɩ̃ õkona.
40012050	Gɩdonɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũu tuur, ɔr dʋɔn ɩ̃ õkuun, na ɩ̃ õkhɛr, na ɩ̃ nɩ.
40013001	Ga wiilera Jeju kɔɔ the cʋɔrɔ a too mɩɩr nɔɔra,
40013002	dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ gbɛbɩ pʋɔraa a der, dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ jʋʋn a too gboroona, sɩ dɩ tibil jɔɔle too mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔra.
40013003	Dɩ a mɩɩ wɛr thɩmɩa jɔɔ na sokpaa. A so warɛ ayɩ:
40013004	Bi jaldaar gɩ, a the da-n jal be. Dɩ mɔna a-n jalnɩ, yɛ̃ bi jire hʋɛra, dɩ 'lominə pɔ ʋʋl.
40013005	Yɛ ji wo bokanana, ka thɩ nʋʋn na jɔrna', a phu dapaara kɔrɔ, gɩdonɩ ga jɩɩ mʋʋ a hulõə'.
40013006	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wire phanɩ, dɩ ɩtʋɛ hẽ, gɩ ɔ̃'ɔlɔnɛ a khi, gɩdonɩ ga yɩ nɛ gɔ paara'.
40013007	Yɛ ji wo ka uu hanɩ, dɩ uu ɩɩr a sɩlã gɩ.
40013008	Yɛ ji thɩ bʋɔra a phu a bɩ̃, bi bɩɛl n bɩnɛ dɩɩ hana be tamaa, ɩkha kpalãther, ɩkha kpelẽ yʋɔr.
40013009	Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
40013010	Dɩ kpãkpãadara tɔr pɔ Jejura a bulee: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa-n mɩɩna wɩ sokpaa?
40013011	Dɩ birse wi: Nɛr Thãgba kɔɔ ha nɩ jɛ thɩ̃ gbulsɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ ƴũ fãgadaar doda, sɩ we wer Thãgba na ha wa'.
40013012	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ thɩ̃ɛ, Thãgba na bire na haa na dɛbɩrɔ, dɩ na hana gɩ dɩ ga jɩɩ jɔr; sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ thɩ̃a', Thãgba na tiirəərerakɛ phubi gɩrɛɛkɛra a hananɩ.
40013013	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ma-n mɩɩna wɩ sokpaa; gɩdonɩ wɩ-n hɩɩnɛ sɩ wa yɩ ga, wɩ-n pɛ nũu sɩ wa-n nɩa', dɩ wa jɩ kɩrʋ dakha ga.
40013014	Dɩ awɩdara Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ thakɛ ayɩ: “Na-n nɩɛrɛ wer bɔɔbɔɔ na anɩ nũ, sɩ na jɩ kɩrʋ kpɩɩraka'. Na-n hɩɩnɛ wer bɔɔbɔɔ na anɩ yi, sɩ na yɩ gɩ kpɩɩraka'.
40013015	Gɩdonɩ tɩbɩlaakɛɛ ha debire a dibi; wɩ sɔbɩrɛ awɩ nũ ka, a khaan dakha awɩ yi, anaa ga hor wa yɩ gɛr na awɩ yi, a na nɩɛ na awɩ nũ, a na jɩna kɩrʋ na awɩ bɩ̃, a na kɛr na bir mar, dɩ mɛr Thãgba na kpɛɛ wɩ.”
40013016	Sɩ gɩ da nar, gɩdonɩ ner n yɩ gɛr dɩ nɩ nɩ gɛr dakha.
40013017	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, Thãgbaa bobona na tɩɩ sarasɔ jɔɔjɔɔ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ yɩ gɩrɛɛkɛra nɩ-n yɩnɩ gɩrɛ, sɩ wa kɔɔ yɩ ga, wɩ nɩɛna dakha gɩrɛɛkɛra nɩ-n nɩɛnɩ gɩrɛ, sɩ wa kɔɔ nɩ ga.
40013018	Dɩ gɛr gɩ nɛrɛ, nɩ pɛ nũu gɩrɛ dɔnɩ bi jal sokpaa kɩrra.
40013019	Ʋrɛ n nɩɛnɛnɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ thɩmɩɩ sɩ aa-n jɩ kɩrʋa', ɔr hʋɔn hʋ nʋɔ ka be kɔɔ jalnɩ, dɩɩ do Satã n pʋɔn, dɩ tiir beele kɔɔ jalanɩ ɔɔ hara.
40013020	Ʋkha n ho boka thɩɩ ka be jalnɩ, a-n nɩɛrɛ Thãgbaa so dɩ tu dapaara na daʋ,
40013021	sɩ aa-n sɩ gar dɩɩ yɩ nɛ gɔ paar ɔɔ hara ga, bɔɔ gbe a-n pər gar dɩbara; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩwɛ na kpoore n danɩ, dɩɩ do Thãgbaa soolera dɔ nɔɔ dɩɩ do dapaara a faarɛ ha pɛrɛ.
40013022	Ʋkha n nɩɛ Thãgbaa so sɩ dɩɩ do a hʋrɛ ka uu hanɩ sɩ be jallɔ, sɩ dɛr bɔɔraakɛra na lẽle thɩ̃ kpɩɛr fifiləle, gele n ɩrɛ dɩɩ sɩlã Thãgbaa so dɩ ga-n puno na se bə'.
40013023	Ʋrɛ n nɩɛnɛnɩ Thãgbaa so dɩ jɩ kɩrʋ, ɔr hʋɔn thɩ bʋɔ ka be kɔɔ jalnɩ dɩɩ do a-n ser be: Bi bɩɛl n ser tamaa, ʋ kpalãther, ʋ kpelẽ yʋɔr.
40013024	Dɩ a so warɛ sokpa kpɩɩ wo ayɩ: Ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ gɩ hurɛ kuunikɛ jalanɩ jʋ bi bʋɔ ɔɔ lɔɔ.
40013025	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla n daarnɩ, ɔɔ lãlaardaar pɔr a jal yaya a pɛr jɔraale sa kɔ̃.
40013026	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ jɔ phuni a ɩ̃ a pemi dɩ ga-n bɩ̃, wɩ yɩrɛ dakha yaya.
40013027	Dɩ cɔdaar kuuni thɔ̃daarsɔ pɔ a bulee: Kɔ̃tɩn, ga do jʋ bi bɔɩ fɩ jal afɩ lɔaa? Sɩ ka yayasɔɔkɛ the le?
40013028	Dɩ birse wi: Lãlaardaar cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛɛle. Dɩ thɔ̃dara bulee, dɩ fɩ-n ƴaalɛ sɩ jala phɩrɛ yayasɔra ya?
40013029	Dɩ birse wi: Kpei, a nɩ yɩ nɩ phɩrɛ yaya, na phɩɩrnanɛ jʋ bɔɩ.
40013030	Nɩ sɛ gar, gɩ gbɛbɩ gɩ khɔ̃ bɩɛlbɩɛl, phaphapha gɩ dana jʋ kha bɔɔ. Dɩ a jʋ kha bɔɔ dã, gɛr ma sor jʋ khara: Nɩ kɔɔ phɩrɛ yaya ɓo a le gɩ dera gbulona gbulona wɩ thii, sa kha jɔ a uro ɩ̃ thʋna.
40013031	Dɩ Jeju so warɛ sokpa kpɩɩ wo ayɩ: Ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ gɩ hʋrɛ seneve bireekɛ kuun kɔɔ gbanɩ a jal ɔɔ lɔɔ.
40013032	Thɩr bireekɛ 'lunoni a jɔ be fɛʋ gɩ, sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a phuni pɩ, a-n kɔ̃tɩnɛ dɩ jɔ thɩr bii fɛʋ dɩ ɩ̃ dɩ do thɩrʋ, dɩ 'lominə n pɔ a na tɛl ɔɔ jɛ̃sɔra.
40013033	Dɩ a so warɛ sokpa kpɩɩ wo ayɩ: Ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ gɩ hʋrɛ tabɩɩrɩkɛ khɛr kɔɔ gbanɩ a mʋʋ buru mɩ̃ nyɔ̃kpõ khaa yẽtherra, phaphapha dɩ buru mɩ̃ boloola fɛʋ bʋ̃.
40013034	Gelesɔ fɛʋ sokpaa Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩna tibil jɔɔle. Aa-n kɔɔ mɩɩna wɩ saagado sokpaa gaaga;
40013035	dɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobon kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ na dã oti gɩ sor: “Sokpaasɔ, mɛr Thãgba na-n mɩɩna. Ma mɩɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ kɔɔ keranɩ kɛkɛkɛ a fʋna thɩ̃ ti bɔɔ.”
40013036	Agɩpɩ Jeju faarɛ tibil jɔɔle sa lõ cʋɔrɔ, dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara tɔr pʋɔraa sa sʋʋraa: Mɩɛnɛ sɩ yayaakɛra hanɩ lɔɔ sokpa kɩr.
40013037	Dɩ birse wi: Ʋrɛɛkɛ jalanɩ jʋ bi bʋɔɔle, mɛr tibili Bikuun gɩ.
40013038	Lɩɛ dʋɔn tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ. Jʋ bi bɔɩ dʋɔn ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩɩ bɩsãsɔ; sɩ yaya dʋɔn puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩ bɩsãsɔ.
40013039	Lãlaardaarɩkɛ jalanɩ, Satã gɩ. Dɩ jʋ kha bɔɔ dʋɔn thɩɩkɛɛ pɩ bɔ. Jʋ khadara dʋɔn Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ.
40013040	Dɩ mɔ̃ wa khɩɩnɩ yaya a na thii, mɛ̃ ga ha thɩ̃ɩkɛɛ pɩ bɔ dakha.
40013041	Mɛ̃ mɛr tibili Bikuun na thɔ̃ ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ, dɩ wa tiir ɩ̃ fãgadaarɩ dɩra wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n cʋɛnɩ tɩbɩla dɩ wa-n bara, na wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ sopugo,
40013042	a na dʋʋrna wɩ dɔɔraakɛ jʋɔnɔnɩ dɩɩ ka bɩnɔ na faa, ka wa bɩnɩ wa-n yɩrna nyɩma.
40013043	Liir dɩphã tɩɩ sarasɔ na-n carã awɩ Thɩ fãgadaarɩ dɩra mɔ̃ wire n caranɩ. Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
40013044	Ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ, gɩ hʋrɛ lẽle thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ keranɩ lɔɔ. Dɩ tibilikɛ yɛ gɩnɩ, a-n kerore sɩ dɩ jal na daʋ, dɩ dolõ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a hananɩ dɩ thena lɩɛɛle.
40013045	Ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ wo, gɩ hʋrɛ ƴaƴabɩdaarɩkɛ hanɩ dɛ ƴaallɔ.
40013046	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a yɩnɩ dɛ bireekɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ ka, a-n jaal dɩ dolõ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a hananɩ dɩ thena dɛ bireele.
40013047	Ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ wo, gɩ hʋrɛ thʋ̃ pherdaakɛ wɩ dʋnanɩ lanyʋɔnna, dɩɩ fʋ thʋ̃ caar dɩɩdɩɩ.
40013048	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ gɩ hini, thʋ̃ pherdara n hallɛ thena gẽgerena, sa too a phiir gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ a pɛ daʋ, sa dʋʋrna gɩrɛ na bʋɔnɔna' a faa.
40013049	Mɛ̃ ga ha thɩɩkɛɛ pɩ bɔ. Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ na ɩna na lee tɩɩ puusɔ tɩɩ sarasɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn,
40013050	sɩ na dʋʋrna wɩ dɔɔraakɛ jʋɔnɔnɩ dɩɩ ka a na faa, ka wa bɩnɩ wa-n yɩrna nyɩma.
40013051	Nɩ jɩrɛ kɩrʋ gɩrɛsɔra fɛʋ dɩphã gaa? Dɩ wɩ tu: Ɔɔ, sɩ jɩrɛ kɩrʋ.
40013052	Dɩ a so warɛ ayɩ: Gɛr gɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar wo jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaarɩkɛ 'lɛnɩ dɩɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ ƴũ fãgadaar doda, a hor cɔdaar kuunikɛ n tenɩ ɔɔ lẽle thɩna thɩ̃ phana na thɩ̃ tɩna.
40013053	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju mɩɩnɩ ga sokpasɔɔkɛ pɩ, gɛr a ɩɩrɔ le a jal.
40013054	Dɩ a kɛrrɛ bir kɔ̃ ɔɔ dʋɔ, a ma da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, dɩ mɛ̃ nʋɔ kpaa wɩ dɩ wa-n so ayɩ: Ka kpɛsɛ caakɛ na nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ caakɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ the?
40013055	Ga do ɔr dʋɔn thɩr khaadaarɩ bikuunaa? Ga do ɔɔ nɩ wɩ-n we Marɩaa? Dɩ ga do Jakɩ, na Jojɛfɩ, na Sɩmɔ̃, na Juudi dɔ ɔɔ õkuunsɔaa?
40013056	Dɩ ɔɔ õkhɛrsɔ fɛʋ wo na ha kha na sɛrɛaa? Dɩ ka a yɩ gelesɔra fɛʋ?
40013057	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ beesuu. Dɩ Jeju so warɛ ayɩ: Paar fɛʋ Thãgbaa bobon na-n 'lee cʋrɛ, saagado ɔɔ dʋɔ na ɔɔ cɔ gaaga.
40013058	Dɩ aa-n cʋʋ le nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ jɔa', gɩdonɩ wa-n pɩɛ haara'.
40014001	Ga bɔɔlera Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar buu kɔɔ nɩɛ mɔ̃ Jejuu i the n kpaarnɩ, a so ɔɔ thɔ̃darara ayɩ:
40014002	Jã Batɩsɩtɩ gɩ, ɔr ɩrɛ a the khirera, gɛr gɩ dɩ puno da-n cʋʋ ga nɔ kpaa thɩ̃sɔɔle.
40014003	Gɩdonɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩra kɔɔ fʋrɛ Jã a li a to khaɩra. A cʋʋrɛ thale gɩ da Ɛrɔdɩadɩraakɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ õkuun Filipii khɛr.
40014004	Gɩdonɩ Jã n kɔɔ sʋʋraarɛ dɩ yɩ: Ga teena dɩ fa tee afɩ õkuuni khɛr na hea'.
40014005	Dɩ a-n ƴaalɛ a kʋʋ, sɩ dɩɩ do tibil jɔ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ maar na-n fʋʋ, gɩdonɩ wɩ-n hɩɩnɛ Jã dɩ do Thãgbaa bobon.
40014006	Sɩ wireekɛ wɩ kɔɔ kɔnɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ, ga wiile daan dɩ wɩ hana fɛtɩ; le Ɛrɔdɩadɩɩ bikhɛr lõ da-n sa bɩna wɩrɛraakɛ wɩ wenɩɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ dar Ɛrɔɔdɩra;
40014007	dɩ mɛ̃ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛ ayɩ, ɩna haarɛ thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a na bɩɛlnɩ.
40014008	Dɩ ɔɔ nɩ kɔɔ tʋɔrɛ pɛr ayɩ ayɛ: Pɛ mɩ kɩɛr dapaara Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ yʋ kpɛ̃kpɛrɛ̃ biro.
40014009	Dɩ haar n kɔɔ helle fãgadaarɩle, sɩ gɩdonɩ ɔɔ ʋlfɛɛle na wɩrɛ a wenɩ fɛtɩra dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ so ayɩ, wɩ hanaa.
40014010	Dɩ a thʋɔn khaɩra dɩ wɩ jal a kʋ Jã a kur yʋʋ.
40014011	Dɩ wɩ gbaar yʋʋra a pɛr kpɛ̃kpɛrɛ̃ biro a pɔna ha khebir, dɩ khebir gba jalna ha ɔɔ nɩ.
40014012	Dɩ Jãa kpãkpãadara pɔr a gba khire a dʋ, sa jal a mɩɛ Jeju.
40014013	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju nɩɛnɩ gele, a faarɛ sa gba gborõo a the le, a jal dɩkhãa pa bəənnə, dɩ tibil jɔ nɩɛrɛ a the dɩɩsɔra a kpaaraa na nɛɛ.
40014014	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n thenɩ gboroona, a yɩrɛ tɩbɩlaale tə̃tə̃tə̃ dɩ wa-n kʋʋ bʋɔ, dɩ a kpɛɛrɛ awɩ khodara.
40014015	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ dʋɔrnɩ, kpãkpãadara tɔr pʋɔraa a sʋʋraa: Paarɩkɛra sɩ hanɩ bəənnə gɩ, dɩ bɔɔ 'lire kar. Bɩlanɛ tibil jɔɔkɛra, wɩ jal dɩ biisɔra, wɩ the dɩkɔ wɩ kho.
40014016	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ga teena wɩ kɔna ga, nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n hana wɩ dɩkɔ wɩ kho.
40014017	Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Sa hana thɩ̃ɛ saagado buru yemɔɩ na thʋma yenyɔ dɩbara gaaga.
40014018	Dɩ a sor: Nɩ gba ɛna ha mɩ.
40014019	Dɩ a sor tibil jɔraalera wɩ tɔɔ ka hʋɔn hanɩ. Dɩ a gbaar buru yemɔɩɩlera na thʋma yenyɔɔle, a gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ sa bɩɛl Thãgba pɛr. Sɩ agɩpɩ, dɩ kuur burura a ha kpãkpãadara, dɩ kpãkpãadara gba tɩnɛ tibil jɔɔle.
40014020	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ khor a hi phi, sɩ wɩ gbaar dakuruukɛ wɩ tɩnɛnɩ sa sɩ, dɩɩ hi kpona yʋɔr yenyɔ.
40014021	Sɩ wɩrɛ kɔɔ khɔnɩ, wɩ thɔɔrɛ kona gbɩlanɩ yemɔɩ, sɩ wa ther khɛra na bɩsana a pɛra'.
40014022	A gele pɩ dapaara, Jeju tɔr ɔɔ kpãkpãadara pɛr, dɩ wɩ lõ gboroona wɩ kʋʋlʋʋ ƴɩɛ wɩ iir gɩ̃ iiro, ɔbɔɔkɛ a na-n bɩlanɩ tibil jɔɔle.
40014023	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a bɩlanɩ tibil jɔɔle pɩ, a gbaar jal jʋʋn gɔ̃gʋɔna dɩbara a bɩɛl Thãgba. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ dʋɔrnɩ, a hale dɩbara.
40014024	Sɩ gborõo 'lire ha mɩɩr nɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ nyʋɔn ubi dɩ ga-n be gborõole, gɩdonɩ jɩɛ wɩ telẽ.
40014025	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ n lɔrnɩ wɩllɛ, Jeju gbaar da-n pɔ ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara da-n ɩɩr mɩɩr nɔ nyʋɔnna ƴũ.
40014026	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ da-n ɩɩr nyʋɔnna ƴũ, maar fʋlɛ wɛr dɩɩ ka, dɩ wɩ sor aa: Khĩdidaar ga do. Dɩ gɩdonɩ maar fʋlɛ wɛr, wɩ mar dɩ wa-n hulẽ.
40014027	Dɩ Jeju so war dapaara ayɩ: Nɩ pɩɛr 'lar mɛr Jeju gɩ, na-n do maar n fʋ na'.
40014028	Dɩ Pɩɛr birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado fɛr gɩ, sɔ mar ɩ̃ ɩɩr dakha mer nyʋɔnna ƴũ ɩ̃ pɔ far.
40014029	Dɩ sʋʋraa: Ɩna. Dɩ Pɩɛr the gboroona a ɩɩr nyʋɔnna ƴũ da-n jal Jejura.
40014030	Sɩ mɔ̃ a yɩnɩ jɩɛ dɩ ga-n the na fãga maar fʋʋrɛ, dɩ a mar da-n mʋʋ nyʋɔnɔ a hulẽ aa: Kɔ̃tɩn, taa mɩ.
40014031	Dɩ dapaara Jeju 'laa nyɔ̃ɔ fʋʋ sa sʋʋraa: Fɛr ha pɛ 'lũdaar, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa-n baalɔ?
40014032	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ lonɩ gboroona jɩɛ kurre.
40014033	Dɩ wɩrɛ hanɩ gboroona pɔr a gburõku, dɩ wa-n fʋɔr Jeju dɩ wa-n sona aa: Sobɔr gɩ, Thãgbaa Bikuun fɩ do waa gel.
40014034	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ iirni iiro pɩ, wɩ jaal a dã Jenejarɛtɩ khʋra.
40014035	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla paarɩlera jɩnɩ Jeju, wɩ thɔnanɛ thɩmɩa paar fɛʋ ga bənəəle. Dɩ wɩ kpar khodarasɔ fɛʋ a pɔnanaa.
40014036	Dɩ wɩ-n phʋʋrʋʋrɛ a ha nɩ hʋɛ ɩna-n thar ɔɔ kẽkẽ nɔrarakɛ dɩbara dɔrɔɔm. Dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ thaaraanɩ, awɩ kho kpɛɛrɛ.
40015001	Le jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ the Jerujalɛm a pɔ Jejuu pa a bulee:
40015002	Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ afɩ kpãkpãadarasɔ na-n kʋɛ asɩ mama kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ so? Gɩdonɩ a wa kho dɩkor, wa-n phʋɔl awɩbara ga.
40015003	Dɩ birse wi: Sɩ nɛrɛ dakha, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n kʋɛ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ dɩɩ do anɩ mama kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ so hɩɩn dɔ kɩrʋ?
40015004	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba sor ayɩ: “Na cɔ afɩ thɩ na afɩ nɩ” dɩ “ado ntɛ nɩɩr ɔɔ thɩ, a ɔɔ nɩ gɩ, wɩ kʋɔ.”
40015005	Sɩ ner n yɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ na sɔnɩ ɔɔ thɩra agɩbo ɔɔ nɩra nayɩ: Thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ ma kɔɔ ha fɩnɩna gɩ bul fi, gɛr mɩ gba dɩɩ do Thãgbaa khaarda;
40015006	wa tibilile na hana a cʋ ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ bã; dɩɩ do mɛ̃ anɩ mama kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ so cʋʋ Thãgbaa so dɩɩ debi do mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ.
40015007	Nɛr bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, sobɔr Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩ kɔɔ so anɩdara ger waa, gɩdonɩ a sor ayɩ:
40015008	“Nɔfaar tibil ca ƴɩrɛ n cʋna mɛr Thãgba pɔɩ, sɩ dɩ awɩ ha hʋnɔna mɩ fĩi.
40015009	Fʋɔrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n fʋɔr mɩnɩ, mɔlɔ gɩ, gɩdonɩ jɔfʋʋkɛ tɩbɩla pɛrnɩ wɩ-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla.”
40015010	Dɩ Jeju wer tibil jɔ dɩ wɩ pɔ dɩ so war: Na-n pɛ nũu a jɛ kɩrʋ.
40015011	Ga do gɩrɛ n lonanɩ tibil nɔɔ, gɛr na cʋgɛɛ dɩ na bisə', sɩ gɩrɛ n kanɩ the tibili nɔɔ, gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ na cʋgɛɛnɩ dɩ na bise.
40015012	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara tɔr pɔ a sʋʋraa: Fɩ jɩrɛ dɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ fɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ dor nɛ baradaa jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarara bɛ?
40015013	Dɩ birse wi: Thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ ɩ̃ Thɩ ƴũ na diirnə', nɛɛ wa phɩɩrna na faa.
40015014	Nɩ sɛ war. Yara wɛ dɩ wa-n thɔɔ yara. Ado yaarʋ na thɔɔ yaarʋ, wɛr yenyɔ fɛʋ na jiire kõkorro.
40015015	Dɩ Pɩɛr bulee: Mɩɛnɛ sɩ sokpaakɛɛ kɩrra.
40015016	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Nɛrɛ dakha, jaa jɩɩr 'lũ ner dakha wo koe?
40015017	Na jɩ gɩ dɩɩ do thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n lonanɩ tibili nɔɔ, bucuurə gɩ-n ka ɓo, sɩ agɩpɩ dɩɩ the cuuəə?
40015018	Sɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ n thɛnɩ tibili nɔɔ gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ n thɛnɩ haarra, dɩ gɛr dɔ gɩrɛra n cʋɛnɩ tibil dɩ bise.
40015019	Gɩdonɩ tibil haarra, le kpɩɛr puu n the, na tɩɩ kʋr, na khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaalɛ na kũu kpɩɩ ƴaalɛ, na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ, na yuur, na sõso so jɩɩr, na tibil i kʋɛrɛ.
40015020	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ tibil dɩ bise, sɩ a fa phʋɔl afɩbara ga, sa kho dɩkor, gele na cʋʋ tibil da bisə'.
40015021	Dɩ agɩpɩ, Jeju the le a jal lõ Tɩɩr na Sɩdɔ̃ khʋra.
40015022	Dɩ hɩnɛ Kanãa khɛr gɩ, a ha ga khʋraalera, a pɔ da-n hulẽ ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun, jɛ mɩ bʋɔra. Ɩ̃ bikhɛr hale dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbuu na-n hʋɔlɔ jɔɔ ka.
40015023	Sɩ Jeju na deeraa nʋɔa', dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara tɔ pɔ a sʋʋraa: Weaa a kɔ̃, gɩdonɩ a-n kɩɛr sɛr nʋɔ khiro kpɛ.
40015024	Dɩ birse wi: Thãgba na thɔ̃ mɩ saagado Ɩjɩrayɛl caraakɛ bureni a ho banaa gaaga.
40015025	Sɩ khɛrɩle pɔr a gburõkuraa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ɩna taa mɩnakɛ.
40015026	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Ga bɔr dɩ fa gba bɩsanaa dɩko na pɛ benana ga.
40015027	Dɩ khɛrɩle bir birsee: Sobɔr gɩ wer Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩ bebe n khorrakɛ dakurusɔɔkɛ awɩ hɩ̃hɩ̃sɔ na-n khonɩ dɩ ga-n jaal le dɩko kho paar thʋnɔ.
40015028	Dɩ le Jeju sʋʋraa: Sobɔr gɩ khɛr, afɩ ha pɛra waa gɩ kɔ̃tɩnɛ. Mɔ̃ fɩ-n ƴaalnɩ, ɔmɛna ga ha. Dɩ wa bɔraalera dɩɩ do ɔɔ bikhɛr kpɛɛrɛ.
40015029	Agɩpɩ Jeju faa paarɩle sa gbana Galile mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔ da-n jal. Dɩ le a jal a jʋʋn gɔ̃gʋɔna a too.
40015030	Dɩ le wo tibil jɔjʋɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃ pʋɔraarɛ na nɛ kʋɛdara, na tãdara, na yarasɔ, na nɔ madarasɔ, na wɩ̃ khodaar kpɩɩ jɔɔ. Dɩ wɩ pɔna wɛr a der ɔɔ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn dɩ a kpɛɛ wɛr.
40015031	Dɩ mɛ̃ nʋɔ kpaa tibil jɔɔle mɔ̃ wɩ yɩnɩ nɔ madara dɩ wa-n mɩɩ thɩmɩa, na tãdara dɩ wɩ kpɛɛna, dɩ nɛ kʋɛdara na-n sa bɔɔbɔɔ, yarasɔ bir wa-n yɩ. Dɩ tibil jɔɔlera n dʋbɩrɛ Ɩjɩrayɛl Thãgbaa i.
40015032	Dɩ Jeju wer ɔɔ kpãkpãadara a so war ayɩ: Bʋɔ fʋ mɛr tibil jɔraakɛ, gɩdonɩ wire yẽther ha gɩrɛ wɩ toona mɩnɩ, sɩ wa hana thɩ̃ɛ na khoa'. Dɩ ma ƴaal ɩ̃ bɩlã wɩ na kɔmɛra' agakpaana ga khabɩ wɛr hʋɛra.
40015033	Dɩ kpãkpãadara sʋʋraa ayɩ: Mɔ̃ sa fʋ sɩ na yɩ kɩɛr dɩkɔ bəənnə thaa, dɩ ga taa bʋɔ dɩ tibil jɔ ca ƴɩrɛ na kho na hi?
40015034	Dɩ Jeju bule wi: Buru yemɔ̃ nɩ hana? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Makonyɔ gɩ na thʋ̃ yɩra ɩkha.
40015035	Dɩ a sor tibil jɔraalera wɩ tɔɔ thʋnɔ;
40015036	agɩpɩ dɩ gba buru makonyɔɔlera na thʋmaalera. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a kuure a ha ɔɔ kpãkpãadarasɔ, dɩ kpãkpãadara gba a tɩnɛ tibil jɔɔlera.
40015037	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ khor a hi phi, sɩ dakurusɔɔkɛ sɛnɩ kpona makonyɔ wɩ kɔɔ gba dɩɩ hi.
40015038	Sɩ wɩrɛ kɔɔ khɔnɩ dɩkɔɔlera, wɩ kɔɔ daan kona gbɩlanɩ yenã, sɩ wa ther khɛra na bɩsana a pɛra'.
40015039	Agɩpɩ dɩ bɩlã dɩphã tibil jɔɔle sa lõ gboroona, a gba da-n jal Magadã khʋra.
40016001	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara, na wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala', pɔr Jejura dɩ wa-n fifiləə a bulee a nɛ nar nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ thãgbara ƴũ.
40016002	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Dʋɔrɔ nɩ-n sor aa, thãgba na pəbire wire, gɩdonɩ ƴũ bɩsɩrɛ.
40016003	Dɩ duuro dɩ nɩ yɩ aa, thãgba na ɩnɛ nĩ, gɩdonɩ ƴũ dor ndɔlɔ̃pa sɛ haar. Nɩ-n punone dɩ nɩ jɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ n hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ, sɩ na-n ka dɩ nɩ puno jɩ jenasɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ bɔɔkɛɛda ga.
40016004	Nĩdaraakɛ puuroni thakɛ, kɛ faanɩ awɩ Thãgba, n ƴaalɛlakɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ, sɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kpɩɩ na bir na yɩ saagado Jonasɩɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ gaaga. Agɩpɩ a faa wɛr sa jal.
40016005	Sɩ kpãkpãadara n kɔɔ iire sa diinə buru gbaar.
40016006	Dɩ Jeju so war ayɩ: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ na-n tɛ̃tɛna jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na halaa taba'.
40016007	Dɩ kpãkpãadara ma dɩ wa-n mɩɩ kha awɩ ha ayɩ: Gɩdonɩ sa kɔɔ gba buruə', gɛr gɩ.
40016008	Dɩ Jeju jɩ mɔ̃ wɩ-n mɩɩnɩ kha a bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n mɩɩ kha anɩ ha, nɛr ha pɛ 'lũdara aa, na kɔɔ gba buruə yaa?
40016009	Jaa na jɩ kɩrʋ paa koe? Na jɩna buru yemɔɩɩkɛ tɩbɩla gbɩlanɩ yemɔɩ kɔɔ khonɩ na kpõ nʋɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ uulnəə?
40016010	Na buru makonyɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla gbɩlanɩ yenã kɔɔ khonɩ na kpõ nʋɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ uulnəə?
40016011	Mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ dɩ na jɩ kɩrʋ pa? Ga do burudaa mɩ mɩɩ na'. Sɩ na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na halaa tabɩra.
40016012	Dɩ le wɩ jɩ dɩphã dɩ mɔ̃ a yɩnɩ wa-n dɔ bʋrɛ, ga do buru cʋʋ tabɩɩr ga, sɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na halaa dɩɩr a so.
40016013	Dɩ mɔ̃ Jeju danɩ Sejare Fihpi khʋra, a bulele ɔɔ kpãkpãadara thɩ̃ɛ thakɛ ayɩwɔɔ: Amɛ tɩbɩla n yɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ka dor?
40016014	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Ɩkha n yɩ, Jã Batɩsɩtɩ fɩ do. Wɛ n yɩ, Elɩ fɩ do. Wɛ n yɩ wo, fɛr dɔ Jeremɩ agɩbo Thãgbaa bobon bɩɛl.
40016015	Dɩ bule wi: Sɩ ner, amɛ nɩ-n yɩ mɩ dor?
40016016	Dɩ Sɩmɔ̃ Pɩɛr birsee: Fɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti Thãgba yidaarɩ Bikuun.
40016017	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Gɩ da farɛ Sɩmɔ̃ Jonasɩɩ bikuun, gɩdonɩ ga do tibil kpɩɛrɛra gɩ the dɩ fɩ jɩ thɩ̃ɛɛka', sɩ ɩ̃ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũ gɩ.
40016018	Sɩ mɛrɛ, mɩ so farɛ: Ga boka kɔ̃tɩnaakɛra ma ɩɩr ɩ̃ we gbɛbɩdara, sɩ fe wer Pɩɛr fa-n do (i kɩrʋ dʋɔn bokaar), dɩ khĩdi dʋɔɔ fãgasɔ na mar na kəə war kpɩɩraka'.
40016019	Ma ha fɛr ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩɩ lakilesɔ, dɩ gɩrɛ fa lini thɩɩra, oti ga li Thãgbaa dʋɔ dakha, sɩ gɩrɛ fa thʋbɩnɩ thɩɩra, oti ga thʋbɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ dakha.
40016020	Dɩ a kpãkpaanɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ, wa-n so tibillə dɩ Kirisiti ha na'.
40016021	Liir Jeju ma dɩphã da-n so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara casɩ, mɔ̃ ɔr teenanɩ a jala Jerujalɛm, kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ n gaarʋʋ jɔɔ, sɩ wɩ kʋʋ dakha, sɩ wire yẽther wirera a na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera.
40016022	Sɩ Pɩɛr kpaarɛ kana pa kpɩɩ, a ma da-n phaanʋʋ ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, Thãgba na thʋ̃ na tu dɩ thɩ̃ɛ tha.e na dã fɩ kpɩɩa'.
40016023	Sɩ Jeju kɛr a so Pɩɛrra ayɩ: Hala mɩ ƴɔɔ Satã. Fɛr dɔ mar nɛ baradaa, gɩdonɩ ga do Thãgbaa kpɩɛr fɩ-n kpɩɛra', sɩ mɔ̃kɛ tibil n kpɩɛrnɩ gɩ.
40016024	Le Jeju so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Ado ntɛ pɛr haar ɩna-n kpa mar, dɔ a faa dɩbara yɩrnanɛ, sɩ a gba ɔɔ kʋkʋ thɩr a na-n kpana mar.
40016025	Gɩdonɩ tibilikɛ n kanɩ dɩ hana bʋ dʋr na ɔɔ yi, ga ka na buurəəre. Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛɛ yi na bonɩ mɛrɛra, ɔr na ka na 'lɛ gɩ waa gel.
40016026	Gɩdonɩ anyee bɔ ca ga taa tibil, ado a 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ, sɩɩ do ɔɔ yi buurəəre? Dɩ agɩbo anye haankɛ dɩ tibi na gba na debina ɔɔ yi?
40016027	Gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na bire na ɩ̃ na ɩ̃ Thɩɩ i dʋbɩ nakha ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ. Liir ma ka tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl thɩ̃ɛ dɩ ga mɩɛna mɔ̃ ntɛɛ thɔna hanɩ.
40016028	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ɩkhasɔ wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩ kɩɛr na khiir, sɩɩ do wa yɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ɔbɔɔkɛ ma-n ɩnɩ ɩ̃ gba fãga gaaga.
40017001	A wire maadõ ka pɩ, Jeju kpar Pɩɛr na Jakɩ na Jã Jakɩɩ õkuun, dɩ wɩ jal kha pa kpɩɩ a jʋʋn gɔ̃gɔ̃ gbaana.
40017002	Dɩ Jejuu tomɩ debire awɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ ɔɔ ƴɛ na-n carbara mɔ̃ wire n carbaranɩ, ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ debi a bulolo phõphõphõ mɔ̃ dahɩrɛ n hanɩ.
40017003	Dɩ hɩnɛ Mʋɩjɩ na Elɩ kɔɔ the warɛ dɩ wa-n khʋɛ kha na Jeju.
40017004	Dɩ Pɩɛr so Jejura: Kɔ̃tɩn, gɩ bɔrɛ sɩ hanɩ kɩɛr. Ado fɩ ture, ma dʋrɛ waa yẽther kɩɛr, bɩɛl n do afɩda, bɩɛl n do Mʋɩjɩɩda, bɩɛl n do Elɩɩda.
40017005	Mɔna a hanɩ mɩɩrɔ, ndɔlɔ̃pa bulo phɩphɩphɩl gbune a thi war. Dɩ hɩnɛ nʋɔ ther le ndɔlɔ̃paarrara ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛra dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, a lõ mer haar kpɛ. Na-n pɩɛ nũu.
40017006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ kpãkpãadara nɩɛnɩ nʋɔɔle, wɩ jiire sumo thɩɩra, gɩdonɩ maar fʋlɛnɛ wɩ jɔɔ ka.
40017007	Sɩ Jeju tɔr dã wɩ a tha war sa so war: Nɩ ɩrɛ, na-n do maar n fʋ na'.
40017008	Dɩ wɩ gbaar ƴɩɛ na hɩɩn, wa yɩ tibil saagado Jeju gɩ dɩbara gaaga.
40017009	Mɔ̃ wɩ thenɩ gɔ̃gʋɔna dɩ wa-n gbũ, Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ thakɛ ayɩ: Na-n gba thɩ̃ɛɛlera nɩ yɩnɩ a mɩɩ tibil bɩɛllaka', phaphapha mɛr tibili Bikuun n ɩɩr ɩ̃ the khirera.
40017010	Dɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ bulele Jeju ayɩ: Dɩ a thale gɩ, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na-n so ayɩ: Elɩ kɔɔ teana a ɩna ɓo?
40017011	Dɩ birse wi: Sobɔr gɩ wer, Elɩ na ɩna na wɛbɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
40017012	Sɩ mɩ so narɛ Elɩ kɔɔ mãa ɩɩn sɩ wa kɔɔ jɩa', sa cʋgʋʋ mɔ̃ wɩ pɛrnɩ haar. Dɩ ɔmɛna wa gaar gɩrɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun.
40017013	Dɩ liir kpãkpãadara jɩ dɩphã dɩ Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩda a mɩɩ wɩ.
40017014	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ danɩ tibil jɔ, kũu bɩɛl pɔr agulẽga Jejura a sʋʋraa:
40017015	Kɔ̃tɩn, jɛ ɩ̃ bikuun bʋɔra, gɩdonɩ ji khidaar gɩ da-n gaar jɔɔ ka. Dɩ wire wire a-n ji dɔɔ na nyʋɔnɔ.
40017016	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ kpaarɛ ha afɩ kpãkpãadara, sɩ wa kɔɔ punoo a kpɛa'.
40017017	Dɩ Jeju birse: Nɛr nĩ babala na puu cʋʋdaraakɛɛ, ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ma thʋ̃ na toona nɩnakɛ gɩ dana? Dɩ ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ma thʋ̃ na fʋ nar haarrarakɛ gɩ dana? Nɩ kpaa ɛna mar kɩɛr.
40017018	Dɩ Jeju mananɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuule dɩ the bɩsaannaale, dɩ dapaara a kpɛɛrɛ.
40017019	Dɩ kpãkpãadara tɔr pɔ Jejura a bulee hɛllɩ ayɩ: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ ser na kɔɔ puno a wee kɔ̃tɛɛbuulera a fa ga?
40017020	Dɩ Jeju birse wi ayɩ: Gɩdonɩ anɩ ha pɛ na kpɛra', gɛr gɩ. Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ado nɩ hananɛ ha pɛrɛ dɩɩ ho seneve bireekɛ n hanɩ fɩɩʋ, na punone na so gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ nayɩ: Ǝlə kɩɛr a jala pal, dɩ a na əlle na jal. Dɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛl na hale dɩ na thʋnɔ kpɩɩraka'.
40017021	[Sɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbu ca ʋrɛ na ha therra na the, saagado Thãgba bɩɛlɛ gɩ na nɔ lirəə ga.]
40017022	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ dɩ wa-n kpaar Galile, Jeju so warɛ ayɩ: Wa fʋrɛ mɛrkɛ dɔnɩ tibili Bikuun na ha tɩbɩla,
40017023	dɩ wa kʋ mɩ, sɩ wire yẽther wirera ma ɩɩrɛ a na the khirera. Dɩ wɩ gbobire jɔɔ ka.
40017024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara danɩ Kapɛrnayʋm dɩɩ, wɩrɛ n gbaannɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ lãpho wer Pɩɛr a bulee ayɩ: Anɩ dɩɩrdaarra, a-n lɩmɩnɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ lãpho bɛ?
40017025	Dɩ birse wi: Ɔɔ, a-n lɩmɩnɛ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Pɩɛr lonɩ cʋɔrɔ, Jeju kɔɔ kʋʋlɛ ƴɩɛ a bulee: Sɩmɔ̃, mɔ̃ fɩ-n kpɩɛr? Fãgadara thɩɩra, anara wɩ-n tee lãpho, dɩ agɩbo anara dʋɔnyɛ̃ n tee war? Awɩ bɩsãsɔra wɛ yaa, kpakpalala wɛ?
40017026	Dɩ birsee: Kpakpalala wɛ. Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dɩ gɛr gɩ, bɩsana na hana lɩmɩnɛ na lɩma'.
40017027	Sɩ mɔ̃ sa cʋʋnɩ sɩ gɩ do sa do war nɛ baradaa ga, jala dɔna thʋ̃ pheru mɩɩr nɔ nyʋɔnɔ, sa hala te caca thʋmɩkɛ fa fʋnɩ. Khɛraa nʋɔ. Fa yɩrɛ le war bireekɛ na dananɩ tɩbɩla yenyɔɔ lãpho lɩmɩ. Te jalana a 'laanɛ ɩ̃da na afɩda.
40018001	Ga bɔɔlera kpãkpãadara tɔ pɔ Jejura, a bulee ayɩ: Amɛ dɔ kɔ̃tɩn a jɔrakɛ fɛʋ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra?
40018002	Le Jeju we bɩsã buu dɩ pɔ dɩ thɩɩnʋʋ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa so:
40018003	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ado na debi a ho bɩsã biə', na lõ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra yuuraka'.
40018004	Gɛr gɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na debanɩ na wur na ho bɩsã buukɛ, ɔr na dɔ kɔ̃tɩn na jɔ fɛʋ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩra,
40018005	dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na teanɩ bɩsã buu ʋrɛɛ khaa kɛ, dɩɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ, mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ a tee.
40018006	Nã kɔ̃tɩ̃ tə̃ə juur tibillə fʋɔrɔ wɩ dʋnanaa wɩ faa lanyɔ̃ hulõ paar, baar gɩrɛɛkɛ a na kanɩ na cʋʋ dɩ bɩsã biikɛ pɛ mɩnɩ haar dɩ bɩɛl na bara.
40018007	Ga puure tɩbɩlala thɩɩra gɩrɛraakɛra nɛ baradaa hanɩkɛ. Nɛ baradaa werrakɛ dɔ ga-n hale, sɩ ga puure tibilləəkɛ n cʋɛnɩ dɩ ga-n hale.
40018008	Ado afɩ nyɔ̃ agɩbo afɩ nɔ do far baradaa, kuro dɔna faa ƴɔɔ. Gɩdonɩ a fɩ 'lɛ yire khorr na nyɔ̃ bɩɛl agɩbo nɔ bɩɛl, gɩ baar nyɛ̃ɛ yenyɔ agɩbo nɛɛ yenyɔɔkɛ fa hananɩ, sɩ wɩ dʋna fɩ wɩ faa khorr dɔɔra.
40018009	Dɩ ado afɩ yi dɔ far baradaa, te dɔna faa ƴɔɔ. A fɩ 'lɛ yire khorr na yi khoroo, gɩ baar yinə yenyɔɔkɛ fa hananɩ sɩ wɩ dʋna fɩ bu paar dɔɔra.
40018010	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ na-n beesi bɩsã biisɔɔkɛ bɩɛllaka'. Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ, awɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ hale Thãgbaa dʋɔ ɩ̃ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũu ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn bɔɔ fɛʋ.
40018011	[Gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ɩnɛ ɩ̃ taa wɩrɛɛkɛ bureni.]
40018012	Mɔ̃ nɩ-n kpɩɛr? Ado tibil hana banaa tamaa dɩ bɩɛl bu, a na sɩ tamaa phe birera gɔ̃gʋɔna sɩ a jal a ƴaal ʋrɛ bonəə?
40018013	Sobɔr mɩ so nar ado a yɩɩ, ga dʋʋraarɛ daʋ a na jɔ tamaa phe bireekɛ na burenə';
40018014	mɛ̃ gɩ, anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩle ƴũ, aa-n tu dɩ bɩsã biikɛ bɩɛllakɛ n buə'.
40018015	Ado afɩ omi cʋʋ sopugo, jala dɩbara a nɩɛraa ɔɔ sopugo. Ado a pɛ fɛr nũu, ga dor fɩ cʋʋrɛ afɩ omi dɩ kɛr bir.
40018016	Sɩ ado aa pɛ fɩ nũə', kpa tibil bɩɛl agɩbo yenyɔ a jalana, dɩ mɛ̃ “sɔɔle ɓibi na gʋʋr mɔ̃ sobɔ so jɩdara yenyɔ agɩbo yẽɩher yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ ha.”
40018017	Dɩ ado a bor wele nũ pɛrɛ, gba gɩ dɩphã a sɔ we gbɛbɩdarara. Dɩ ado a bor we gbɛbɩdara nũ pɛrɛ, dɔ dɩphã a ho far thilaar na war gbadaar.
40018018	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na lini kɛ thɩɩra, ɔmɛ̃ ga li Thãgbaa dʋɔ. Sɩ thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na thʋbɩnɩ kɛ thɩɩra, ɔmɛ̃ ga thʋbɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
40018019	Sobɔr mɩ so nar wo, ado tɩbɩla yenyɔ nɛrɛra na tu kha nɔ bɩɛl kɛ thɩɩra, thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩɛnaakɛ wa bɩɛlnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩraakɛ hanɩle ƴũ, a na ha wɛr.
40018020	Gɩdonɩ kãkɛ tɩbɩla yenyɔ yẽthersɔ gbɛbɩnɩ kha na ɩ̃ i, le mɩ-n ha awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
40018021	Le Pɩɛr tɔ dã a bulee ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado ɩ̃ omi cʋʋ mɩ puure, balamɔ̃ ma faa na haa? Nyɛ̃be makonyɔ ga dã ya?
40018022	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Ga do nyɛ̃be makonyɔ mɩ so fara', sɩ nyɛ̃be makonyɔ der paar kpalãther yʋɔr mɩ so.
40018023	Gɛr gɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ, gɩ hʋrɛ fãgadaarɩkɛ ƴaalɛnɩ a ther war ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔɔ pa a hɩɩn.
40018024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a manɩ da-n ther, wɩ kpar tibil bɩɛlɩkɛ hanaanɩ helu gbɩlanɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ der paar gbɩlanɩ a pɔnanaa.
40018025	Dɩ mɔ̃ aa hananɩ thɩ̃ɛ a na lɩma', ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ yɩ dɩ wɩ dolonee, ɔr na ɔɔ khɛr, na ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ, na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a hananɩ a lɩma heluulera.
40018026	Dɩ thɔ̃daarɩle jire a gburõku ɔɔ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa sʋʋraa: Fɔ haar sɩ ma lɩmɩ fɛr fɛʋ.
40018027	Dɩ bʋɔ fʋrɛ thɔ̃daarɩlee kɔ̃tɩna, dɩ faa helula a haa, sa sɩɩraa dɩ jal.
40018028	Mɔ̃ thɔ̃daarɩlera gbanɩ da-n jal, a caananɛ ɔɔ 'walãkha bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n donanɩ kha thɔ̃ bɩɛl, kɛ hanaanɩ dakha helu war be yenãsɔ. Dɩ a fʋʋrɛ a khɩmɩ ulebire sa so: Lɩma mɩ heluukɛ fɩ hana mɩnɩ.
40018029	Dɩ ɔɔ 'walãkhaale jire ɔɔ ƴɛra da-n phʋʋrʋʋ ayɩ: Fɔ haar sɩ ma lɩmɩ fɛr.
40018030	Sɩ a bor sa jalnaa a to khaɩra phaphapha dɩ lɩmʋʋ ɔɔ hella.
40018031	Ɔbɔɔkɛ ɔɔ 'walãkhasɔ yɩnɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛle danɩ thale, bʋɔ fʋlɛ wɛr jɔɔ ka. Dɩ wɩ gbaar gɩrɛɛkɛ dananɩ fɛʋ a jalna a mɩɛ awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃.
40018032	Le kɔ̃tɩn wɩɩ dɩ pɔ dɩ sʋʋraa: Eɛr thɔ̃daar puu, mɩ kɔɔ faarɛ afɩ hel fɛʋ a ha fɩ, gɩdonɩ fɩ kɔɔ phʋʋr mɛr.
40018033	Dɩ fɛrɛ dakha ga teena fɩ jɛ ʋrɛ nɩ donanɩ kha 'walãkha tibil thɔmana bʋɔra, mɔ̃ mɩ kɔɔ jɩ fɩnɩ bʋɔra gaa?
40018034	Dɩ nĩkhii fʋrɛ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle, dɩ gbaa 'laa gardɩ hɔ̃hɔlala wɩ hʋɔlaa phaphapha a bir a lɩmɩ dakha ɔɔ hella fɛʋ.
40018035	Thale ɩ̃ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ ƴũ na cʋʋ na nɛrɛ, ado nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl yɩ, na-n faa anɩ omii dɩ pa na haar fɛʋ a na haa ga.
40019001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju mɩɩnɩ thɩmɩaakɛ dɩɩ pɩ, a ther Galile a jal Jude khʋra, Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩr iiro.
40019002	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃ kɔɔ kpaaraarɛ, dɩ le a kpɛɛ wɩ khoo.
40019003	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ pʋɔraarɛ dɩ wa-n fifiləə ayɩ: Hʋɛ hale dɩ tibil na faa ɔɔ khɛr gãgã dɔɔraakɛrakɛ a yɩɩraanɩ ya?
40019004	Dɩ birse wi: Na kɔɔ yɩɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra, dɩ “kuun na khɛr thɩ̃ Tidaar kɔɔ cʋʋ caca fʋ paaraa”?
40019005	Mee a kɔɔ sor ayɩ: “Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ kuun na lee kha na ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ, sɩ a ɓã kha na ɔɔ khɛr, wɛr yenyɔ n gbɛbɩ wɩ do tibil bɩɛl.”
40019006	Gɩ do mɛ̃ wa do yenyɔ bã, sɩ wɩ coore kha a do bɩɛl. Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba coornɩ dɩɩ do bɩɛl, tibil na-n lee ga.
40019007	Dɩ wɩ bulee wo ayɩ: Dɩ a thale gɩ, mɔ̃gɩdo sɩ dɩ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ 'laa hʋɛ ayɩ: “Kuun n hana ɔɔ khɛr he kuur sɛbɛ sa weaa a faa?”
40019008	Dɩ birse wi ayɩ: Anɩdara khiinoni dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ 'laa hʋɛ nɩ wea anɩ khɛrsɔ na faa. Sɩ caca fʋ paar, ga kɔɔ ha thaka'.
40019009	Sɩ mɩ so narɛ, tibil wo tibilikɛ na faanɩ ɔɔ khɛr, sɩ ga do kũn kpɩɩ ƴaalɛ ga, sa bir he khɛ kpɩɩ, khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaal sopugo a cʋʋ.
40019010	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara sʋʋraa aa: Dɩ ado thale thɩɛna na ha kuun na khɛrra, gɩ baarrakɛ dɩ tibil na he khɛra'.
40019011	Dɩ birse wi: Tɩbɩla fɛʋ na tu thɩmɩɩrɩka', sɩ wɩrɛ dɩbara wɩ hanɩ punone.
40019012	Gɩdonɩ wɛ hale kɛ awɩ nɩsɔ kɔnɩnakɛ dɩ wɩ do kʋ̃bʋʋ, sɩ wɛ hale wo kɛ tɩbɩla cʋʋnɩ dɩ wɩ do kʋ̃bʋʋ. Wɛ hale wo ƴũ fãgadaar doda donɩ nɔɔ dɩ wɩ too kpakpaar. Gɛr gɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ punoneni a na tu thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ, a to.
40019013	Dɩ tɩbɩla kɔɔ gbaar bɩsã bii a pɔna Jejura a dɛɛnɛ war nyɛ̃ɛ sa bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba pɛ war. Sɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ phaanɛ wɩrɛ pɔna wɩnɩ.
40019014	Dɩ Jeju sor: Nɩ dɔ bɩsã bii na-n ɩ̃ mar, na-n pɩɛr Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ hɔnɩ bɩsana, wɛr ƴũ fãgadaar do mana.
40019015	Dɩ a dɛ̃ɛ warɛ nyɛ̃ɛ sa the le a jal.
40019016	Le tibil bɩɛl tɔ pɔ a bule Jeju ayɩ: Dɩɩrdaar, anye dɔ thɩ̃ bʋɔɔkɛ teananɩ ɩ̃ cʋɛ a 'lɛ yire khorr?
40019017	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa-n bule mi gɩrɛraakɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ? Bɩɛl dɩbara haanle kɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ. Ado fɩ-n ƴaalɛ fɩ 'lɛ yire khorr, na hɩnɛ Thãgbaa jɔfʋsɔ.
40019018	Dɩ bulee: Gɩmɔ̃ɔ jɔfʋ? Dɩ Jeju birsee aa: “Fa-n kʋ tibilə', fa-n hana khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n hana kũu kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n yuə', fa-n sõso pɛ tibilə',
40019019	na cɔ afɩ thɩ na afɩ nɩ, dɩ na na dakha afɩ 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara.”
40019020	Dɩ daɓolbirile sʋʋraa: Mɩ kɔɔ mãa nɩ ga jɔfʋraale fɛʋ nũu, anye sɛ mɩ cʋʋrɛra 'lo?
40019021	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Ado fɩ-n ƴaalɛ fɩ bʋɔnɔ a ka, jala dolone gɩrɛ fɩ hananɩ, a gba hana bɔdara, dɩ mɛ̃ fa 'lɛ lẽle thɩ̃ɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, agɩpɩ fɩ ɩ̃ fa-n kpa mar.
40019022	Ɔbɔɔkɛ daɓolbirile nɩɛnɩ ga thɩmɩɩle, a gbure ƴɩɛ da-n kɔna, gɩdonɩ lẽledaar gɩ na sobɔr.
40019023	Dɩ Jeju so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ƴũ fãgadaar dɩ lʋʋn khɩɩrɛ lẽlera.
40019024	Mɩ bire ma-n 'loro wo: Nyɔɔmɛɛ lõokɛ a na lonɩ mɩsɩmɩ kaarra, ka yɔɔrɛ jɔ lẽlee Thãgba fãgadaar dɩ lõ.
40019025	Mɔ̃ kpãkpãadara nɩɛnɩ gele, nʋɔ kpaa wɛr jɔɔ ka, dɩ wa-n so ayɩ: Dɩ a thale gɩ, amɛ na punonenakɛ a na 'lɛ taarɛ?
40019026	Dɩ Jeju hɩɩn wɩ sa so war: Ado tɩbɩlala wer gɩ, thɩ̃ punonaa ga, sɩ Thãgba wer, ɔr n punone thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
40019027	Le Pɩɛr gba thɩmɩa a sʋʋraa: Dɩ hɩnɛ, sɛrɛ sɩ faarɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ sɩ sa-n kpa far, anye sa yɩrɔ gɩrɛ kper?
40019028	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ado mɛr tibili Bikuunna gɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ thɩ̃ɛ na birni na wɛbɩ ga-n do daphaa, dɩ ma too ɩ̃ i dʋbɩ too paraakɛ dɔnɩ fãga too paar, nɛrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ kpaanɛ marnɩ na toore dakha fãga too pa yʋɔr yenyɔra, sɩ na-n kɩɩlna Ɩjɩrayɛl ca yʋɔr yenyɔ.
40019029	Dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ ɩ̃ i na donɩ nɔɔ dɩ na faarɔ ɔɔ cɔ, a ɔɔ õkuunsɔ wɛ, a ɔɔ õkhɛrsɔ wɛ, a ɔɔ thɩ gɩ, a ɔɔ nɩ gɩ, a ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ wɛ, a ɔɔ lɛ gɩ, a na 'lɛr thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ a na 'lɛna yire khorr dakha.
40019030	Sɩ tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ ƴɛ kʋla, wɛr na fien na do sɩka pɩra, sɩ sɩka pɩra jɔɔ n fi wɩ do ƴɛ kʋla.
40020001	Gɩdonɩ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ gɩ hʋrɛ cɔdaar kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ thɛnɩ cʋɔrɔ duuro phiphiphi, da-n ƴaal thɔ̃ dona a pɛr ɔɔ lɔɔ.
40020002	Dɩ wɩ gʋʋrɛ kha na thɔ̃ donaale dɩɩ do a na ha wɛr wi bɩɛl thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ lɩmɩ, agɩpɩ dɩ thɔ̃ wɩ ɔɔ lɔɔ.
40020003	Dɩ a ther khɛ yɔ kpãa bɔɔ a yɩ wɩ̃ tibil, dɩ wɩ too ƴatɔɔ mɔlɔ.
40020004	Dɩ so war: Nɛrɛ dakha, nɩ jala ɩ̃ lɔɔ, agɩpɩ ma ha nɛr gɩrɛɛkɛ na teana nɩnɩ.
40020005	Dɩ wɩ jal. Dɩ a bire the wo ʋlkhɔɔ na mɔ̃ wire ɩnɩ da-n dʋɔr a cʋʋ ɔmɛna wo.
40020006	Dɩ dʋɔrɔ a bire the wo a yɩ wɩ̃ tibil ɩkhasɔ dɩ wɩ too, dɩ bule wi. Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nɩ too kɩɛrra dɩ wire na-n pɩna, sɩ na-n do thɔma ga.
40020007	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Tibil na gba sɩ thɔma ga, gɛr gɩ. Dɩ a so warɛ: Nɛrɛ dakha, nɩ jala ɩ̃ lɔɔ.
40020008	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wire n lonɩ, cɔdaar kuunilera hɩnanɩ lɩɛra sor ɔɔ thɔ̃daraa hɩɩndaarra ayɩ: Wɛ thɔ̃ donana a lɩma wɩ awɩ war, sɩ kɔɔ fɔna sɩka pɩra a danana ƴɛ kʋla.
40020009	Wɩrɛ kɔɔ jalanɩ thɔmana dʋɔrɔ, wɛr bɩɛlbɩɛl 'lɛr wi bɩɛl thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ lɩmɩna oti.
40020010	Dɩ ƴɛ kʋla pɔr pɩpɩɩ paar dɩ wa-n kpɩɛr waa, ɩna 'lɛr jɔɔ, sɩ wɛr bɩɛlbɩɛl dakha 'lɛr wi bɩɛl thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ lɩmɩna oti.
40020011	Dɩ mɔ̃ wɩ 'lɛnɩ thale, wɩ ɩɩrnanɛ khʋ̃ɛ cɔdaar kuunnaale dɩ wa-n so ayɩ:
40020012	Wɩrɛ pɩrɔnɩ a ɩ̃ a cʋʋ lɩɛr bɩɛl dɩbara, fɩ hɩɩn wɛr dɩɩ ka mãkhana sɛrkɛ vɔɔnɩ thɔmana, dɩ ɩtʋɛ be sɩ dakha ga do kpãkpalã ga.
40020013	Dɩ birse tibil bɩɛl wɛrra: Ɩ̃ kuun wei, ma dɩ far fɩɩʋraka'. Ga do mɔ̃ sɩ gʋʋrnɩ kha fɩ kɔɔ ture wi bɩɛl thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ lɩmaa?
40020014	Gba gɩrɛ dɔnɩ afɩda a kɔna. Mɛr ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ ha ʋrɛ dɔnɩ sɩka pɩr mɔ̃kɛ mɩ ha fɩnɩ.
40020015	Ma hana hʋɛ na cʋʋna ɩ̃ thɩ̃sɔ mɔ̃kɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnaa? Agɩbo fɩ-n bel mer gɩdonɩ mɩ hananɛ ha bulo filɛ ya?
40020016	Dɩ Jeju so war ayɩ: Mɛ̃ sɩka pɩra na fi na do ƴɛ kʋla, sɩ ƴɛ kʋla n fi wɩ do sɩka pɩra.
40020017	Mɔ̃ wɩ hanɩ hʋɛra dɩ wa-n jal Jerujalɛm, Jeju kpar kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ dɩ wɩ ha kha pa kpɩɩ, dɩ le hʋɛrara a so war ayɩ:
40020018	Nɩ hɩnɛ, Jerujalɛm sɩ-n jal gɩrɛ, ka wa fʋnɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na ha bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ, dɩ wa pɛ mar so kʋnanɛ,
40020019	sɩ na gba mɩ na ha ca kpala, dɩ wa mãa mɛr, wa ciil mer dakha na khasa, sɩ wɩ gba mɩ wɩ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra. Sɩ wire yẽther wirera ma ɩɩrɛ na the khirera.
40020020	Le Jebedee bikonaa nɩ pɔ na ɔɔ bikuunsɔ a gulẽga sa bɩɛl Jejura dɩkha.
40020021	Dɩ bulee ayɩ: Anye fɩ-n ƴaal? Dɩ birse Jeju: A fɩ gba fãga, 'laanɛ hʋɛ dɩ ɩ̃ bikona yenyɔɔkɛ bɩɛl n too afɩ nyɔ̃bɔra, bɩɛl n too afɩ nyɔ̃bɩlana.
40020022	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Na jɩ gɩrɛ nɩ-n bɩɛlna'. Na punone na yɔ thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ bɔ gaarɛɛkɛ ma yɔnɩ ya? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Ɔɔ, sa punone.
