40020023	Dɩ a bire birse wi wo: Sobɔr gɩ wer, na punone na yɔna ɩ̃ thɩ̃ yɔnada. Sɩ ado ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔ toora gɩ, na ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɩlã toora, ga do ɩ̃ pa gɩ ha dɩ ma 'laa hʋɛa', sɩ wɩrɛ dɩbara ɩ̃ Thɩ gbɛbɩrɔnɩɩda gɩ.
40020024	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ kpãkpãadara yʋɔrɩle kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ gele, nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr õkona yenyɔraale.
40020025	Dɩ Jeju we wer dɩ wɩ pɔ, dɩ so war ayɩ: Nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ ca kpalaa fãgadara n ʋʋnɛ tɩbɩlala kpɛ, dɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩna n cʋʋ warɛ fãga dɩɩ pho ka.
40020026	Sɩ na-n ka jɩna mɛ̃ gɩ ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩna'. Sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩnɩ-n dɔ kɔ̃tɩn, dɔ ɔr n ka a do anɩ thɔ̃daar.
40020027	Sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩnɩ-n dɔ ƴɛ kʋl anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɔ ɔr n ka a do anɩ dee.
40020028	Dɩ mɛ̃ mɛr tibili Bikuun ɩ̃, ga do dɩ tibil na do mar thɔma ga, sɩ mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ ka ɩ̃ do thɔma ɩ̃ 'laana ɩ̃ yi gɩ birse tɩbɩla bərəəm.
40020029	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n thenɩ Jeriko, tibil jɔjʋɔ bərəəm kɔɔ kpar Jejura.
40020030	Dɩ yara yenyɔ kɔɔ hale a too hʋ nʋɔra. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do Jeju n ka, wɩ mar dɩ wa-n hulẽ ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun, jɛ sɩ bʋɔra.
40020031	Dɩ tibi. jɔɔle mana wɛr ayɩ, wɩ pɩra. Sɩ wɩ bire jɩɩ hulẽ kheu ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun, jɛ sɩ bʋɔra.
40020032	Dɩ Jeju jɩɩl sa we wɩ a bule wi: Anye nɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋɛ nar?
40020033	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, asɩ yi sɩ-n ƴaal gɩ khɛra.
40020034	Dɩ bʋɔ fʋ Jeju dɩ tha awɩ yirə, dɩ dapaara dɩ wɩ bir yɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
40021001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n wɔrɔnɩ Jerujalɛm a dã Bɛtɩfaje khʋra, gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔkɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra, le Jeju thɔ̃ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yenyɔ a so war:
40021002	Nɩ jala dɩɩraakɛ nɩ pɛnɩ ƴɩɛ. Na yɩrɛ dapaara kũkə̃ nɩɩ dɩ wa li na daɓolʋ. Nɩ thʋba a kpa wɩ ɛna ha mɩ.
40021003	Dɩ a tibil bule ni thɩ̃ɛ, nɩ sʋɔraa ayɛ: Kɔ̃tɩn n ƴaalɛ; dɩ dapaara a na sɩ warɛ dɩ na kpa na ɩna.
40021004	Dɩ thɩ̃ɛ thakɛ daan gɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobon sonɩ gɩ ha oti.
40021005	“Nɩ sɔ Sɩyɔ̃dara ayɛ: Nɩ hɩnɛ anɩ fãgadaar n pɔr nɛrɛra. Hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ hiirəəre dɩ jʋʋnna kũkə̃ nɩɩ, kũkə̃ ɓolʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ thɔ̃ do nʋmɩ bi.”
40021006	Dɩ kpãkpãadara jaal a cʋʋ gɩrɛ Jeju yɩnɩ wɩ cʋɛ.
40021007	Dɩ wɩ kpar kũkə̃ nɩrɛ na daɓolʋ a pɔna, a gba awɩ kẽkẽsɔ a dɛ̃ɛ war, sa cʋʋ Jeju dɩ jʋʋn.
40021008	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ n belle awɩ kẽkẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ dɩ wa-n pɛ hʋɛra, sɩ wɛ cɩ thɩr jɛ̃ɛ dɩ wa-n pɛ hʋɛra.
40021009	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle kʋʋlɛ Jeju ƴɩɛ, wɛ na-n kpaan khiro, dɩ wa-n hulenasɔ ayɩ: “Ojana, Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun. Bɔnanɛ n hana ʋrɛraakɛ n ɩnanɩ gɩrɛ na Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i. Ojana thãgbara ƴũ pər.”
40021010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju lonɩ Jerujalɛm, dɩɩ fɛʋ kɔɔ tutugore, dɩ wa-n bule ayɩ: Amɛɛ tibil ca ha olela ya fɛ?
40021011	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle birse wi ayɩ: Jeju Thãgbaa bobon gɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Najarɛtɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Galile dɩɩ.
40021012	Dɩ Jeju lʋʋn Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna. A weele wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n dolonenɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔ, na wɩrɛ n thɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ, a tʋɔrna war debidarasɔɔ tabalsɔ a kpɛɛ, na kʋlã puu dolõdaraa too pasɔ,
40021013	sa so war: Mee gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Mɛr Thãgbaa cɔ wa-n we mɛr Thãgbaa fʋɔr pa”, sɩ dɩ ne wer cʋʋ gɩ dɩɩ do yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaraa wɔ̃ pa.
40021014	Dɩ yarasɔ na nɛ kʋɛdara pɔr le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, dɩ Jeju kpɛɛ wɩ.
40021015	Sɩ nĩkhii fʋlɛlɛ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ mɔ̃ wɩ yɩnɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔɔle a-n cʋʋnɩ, na mɔ̃ bɩsanasɔ n huleni le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ ayɩ:
40021016	Ojana, Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun. Dɩ wɩ buleele: Fɩ nɩɛrɛ gɩrɛra wɩ-n sonɩɩ? Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ɔɔ, mɩ nɩɛrɛ. Sɩ a bire bule wi: Na kɔɔ yɩ ga thɩmɩɩ caakɛra Thãgbaa sɛbɛra kpɩɩaa ya? Mee gɩ sor: “Fɛr Thãgba n teere khɩɩrɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ bɩsã yɩrasɔ na ilẽ mamasɔɔ nɔra.”
40021017	Agɩpɩ a faa wɛr sa the dɩɩra a jal Betanɩ, kãkɛ a cɔnɩ.
40021018	A dɩɩ kɔɔ wɩl, mɔ̃ Jeju kɛrnɩ da-n bir le dɩɩra, kɔmɛr fʋʋrɛ.
40021019	Dɩ mɔ̃ a yɩnɩ thɩr khonanɛ hʋɛra, a gbaar pɔ, sɩ aa yɩɩraa thɩ̃a', fa haar gɩ dɩbara. Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju so thɩrʋʋlera ayɩ: Fa se yuurakɛ bã. Dɩ dapaara thɩrʋʋle khi.
40021020	Mɔ̃ kpãkpãadara yɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ thale, nʋɔ kpaa wɛr dɩ wɩ so aa: Mɔ̃ thɩrʋʋle fʋ sa khi dapaara thale ya fɛ?
40021021	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ado nɩ hananɛ ha pɛrɛ sɩɩ do na-n baalɔa', ga do gɩrɛ dananɩ thɩrʋʋkɛ dɩbara na cʋa', sɩ adorakɛ na so gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ ayɩ: Ǝlə kɩɛr a je pal lanyʋɔnna ga cʋʋrɛ.
40021022	Dɩ thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na bɩɛlnɩ Thãgbara na ha pɛrɛ, na yɩ gɛr.
40021023	Dɩ Jeju gbaar jal lõ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a hanɩ da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na tɩbɩlaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ pɔr a bulee ayɩ: Ka hʋ caakɛra fɩ hananɩ dɩ fa-n cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛra the, dɩ amɛ hana fɩ hʋɛɛkɛra?
40021024	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ma bule ner mer dakha thɩ̃ bɩɛl. Ado nɩ birse mi, mɛrɛ dakha ma so narɛ hʋ ca ʋrɛ mɩ hananɩ, dɩ ma-n cʋʋna thɩ̃ ca gɩrɛsɔra.
40021025	Jãa yɔ kpɛɛ, ka gɩ the? Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ yaa, tɩbɩlaa pa gɩ the? Dɩ wɩ mar dɩ wa-n bana kha awɩ hasɔ ayɩ: Ado sɩ tu wo ayɩ: Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ the, a na bule ser nayɩ, dɩ anye dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ sa kɔɔ pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haara?
40021026	Dɩ ado sɩ tu wo ayɩ: Tɩbɩlaa pa gɩ the, sa 'lɛr sor na tibil jɔɔkɛ gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ kɔɔ gbaar Jã dɩ do Thãgbaa bobon.
40021027	Dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ birse Jeju: Sa ja'. Dɩ a so warɛ dakha ayɩ: Dɩ a thale gɩ, ma so nar mer ka mɩ yɩnɩ hʋɛ dɩ ma-n cʋʋna ga thɩ̃sɔɔka'.
40021028	Mɔ̃ nɩ-n kpɩɛr? Kũu bɩɛl gɩ a kɔɔ hana bikona yenyɔ, dɩ a sor cacadaarra ayɩ: Ɩ̃ bɩsã, jala nĩ lɔɔ a kʋlɛ mɩ.
40021029	Dɩ birsee: Ma jala'; agɩpɩ dɩ debi kpɩɛrɛ sa jal.
40021030	Dɩ bir so balanyɔdaarra ɔmɛna. Dɩ birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, ma jaal, sɩ aa jala'.
40021031	Wɛr yenyɔraale, ʋmɔ̃ cʋɛ ɔɔ thɩɩ tuur? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Cacadaar gɩ. Dɩ Jeju so war ayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, war gbadara na bɔdɛlasɔ, wɛr fien kʋʋl nɩ ƴɩɛ dɩ wa-n lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
40021032	Gɩdonɩ Jã kɔɔ ɩnɛ anɩ pa a nɩ nar fɩl sar hʋɛ, sɩ na kɔɔ pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haara'; sɩ war gbadara na bɔdɛlasɔ wɛr pɩɛr ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haar, sɩ nɛrkɛ kanɩ yɩ gɩ, na debirakɛ haar pɩpɩɩ paar sa pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haara'.
40021033	Nɩ pɛ kɛ sokpa kpɩɩ nũu wo. Cɔdaar kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ cʋʋ nãkʋɔr a bã dãgbol diiro, a kpena dakha bi cɔrɔ paar sa mɩ bɛbɛr cɔ gbãa. Agɩpɩ dɩ gba nãkʋɔr hɩɩndara a pɛr wa-n hɩnɛ ɓo, sa gba jal kpaar paar.
40021034	Ɔbɔɔkɛ gɩ ɩnɩ dã bi khʋ̃ bɔɔ, a thʋɔn ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔ wɩ jala nãkʋɔr hɩɩndarara, a tea war nãkʋɔr thɩr be a pɔna.
40021035	Sɩ nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaraalera fʋlɛlɛ thɔ̃daraale, a bɩɩr bɩɛl sa kʋ bɩɛl wo, sa dʋʋrna bɩɛl bokana.
40021036	Dɩ a bire thɔ̃ wɩ̃ thɔ̃dara dɩ wɩ jɔ cacadaraale, sɩ nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaraalera cʋʋ wɛr otirə wo.
40021037	Pɩpɩɩ paar dɩ thɔna war dɩphã ɔɔ bikuun sa so: Wa cʋrɛ ɩ̃ bikuun.
40021038	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaraale 'laanɩ yɩ bikuun, wɩ mɩɩrɛ kha awɩ ha ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ na dʋɔn thɩ̃ hɩn, nɩ dɔ sɩ kʋʋ, sɩɩ do sɛr hɩna thɩɛna.
40021039	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ fʋʋ a dʋna nãkʋɔr khuirə sa kʋʋ.
40021040	Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã, ado nãkʋɔr kɔ̃tɩn pɔ, anye a na cʋʋ nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaar ca wele?
40021041	Dɩ wɩ birsee ayɩ: A na kʋʋrɛ te puule sɩ bʋɔ na fʋʋa', sɩ a gba nãkʋɔr a ha nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaar kpɩɩsɔ wo, kɛ na khʋnanɩ be wa-n haa ɔbɔɔkɛ ga ɩnɩ ga-n se.
40021042	Dɩ Jeju so war: Na kɔɔ hɩɩn gɩrɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ yuuəə ya? Mee gɩ sor ayɩ: “Bokaarɩkɛ cɔ mɛ kɔɔ bonɩ debire a do go tɩ bokaar. Sɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ pa thɩ̃ɛɛlera the, dɩ sɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ do sar thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ.”
40021043	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so nar ayɩwɔɔ: Thãgba na taa narɛ ɔɔ fãgadaarɩ dɩ na ha caarɩkɛ na-n sɩɛnnɩ beekɛ na dɔnɩ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩda.
40021044	[Dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na jenɩ bokaarraalera a na khaarɛ; sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ bokaarɩlera na jironi ga cʋ̃banʋʋnɛ pɛrɛ pɛrɛ pɛrɛ.]
40021045	Ɔbɔɔkɛ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ bu dʋdarasɔ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ sokpaasɔɔle, wɩ jɩrɛ dɩ wɛr Jeju kɔɔ so.
40021046	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ hʋɛ wɩ fʋʋra, sɩɩ do maar kɔɔ fʋɔn wɩ tibil jɔraale, gɩdonɩ wɩ gbaar Jeju dɩ do Thãgbaa bobon.
40022001	Dɩ Jeju bire gba thɩmɩa wo da-n mɩɩna wɩ na sokpaa ayɩ:
40022002	Yũ fãgadaar do, gɩ hʋrɛ fãgadaarɩkɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ fɛtɩ ɔɔ bikuuni herra.
40022003	Agɩpɩ a thʋɔn ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔ wɩ jala wɛ wɩrɛ wɩ kɔɔ soronɩ wɩ pɔ he fɛtɩrara, sɩ wa kɔɔ tu na pɔa'.
40022004	Dɩ a bire thɔ̃ thɔ̃daar kpɩɩsɔ wo a so war ayɩ: Nɩ sɔ wɩrɛrara wɩ wenɩ ayɛwɔɔ: Nɩ hɩnɛ, mɩ gbɛbɩrɛ he fɛtɩ dɩkorra pɩ, mɩ kʋʋrɛ nakena, a kʋʋrna nʋ̃ ƴɩkhasɔ wa khʋɔn kpãkpalã ga; thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ, nɩ ɩna he fɛtɩrara mɛ̃.
40022005	Sɩ wa thernanakɛ werɩle wɩ we wɩna'; sɩ ʋ n gbaar da-n jal ɔɔ lɔɔ, ʋ n gba da-n jal ɔɔ ƴabɩ pa.
40022006	Sɩ wɛ fʋ thɔ̃dara a hʋɔlɔ sa kʋʋr wɩ.
40022007	Dɩ nĩkhii fʋrɛ fãgadaarɩle dɩ thɔ̃ ɔɔ sɔrasɩsɔ, dɩ wɩ bũburõ tɩɩ kʋʋrdaraalera sa thii wi dɩɩ.
40022008	Dɩ agɩpɩ a sor ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔrara ayɩ: Gɩdonɩ he fɛtɩ dɩkɔ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ, sɩ wɩrɛ wɩ kɔɔ wenɩ dɩ ga do wɩ teena gɛra',
40022009	gɛr gɩ, nɩ jala hʋ lee paarsɔ a wɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ nɩ yɩnɩ, wɩ ɩ̃ he fɛtɩra.
40022010	Dɩ thɔ̃daraale ɩɩr jal hʋɛsɔrara a khɩɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ yɩnɩ, tɩɩ puusɔ na tɩɩ bɔɩsɔ, dɩ welela wɩ wenɩ a pɔna wɩ hire he dɩko kho paar.
40022011	Dɩ fãgadaarɩle lʋʋn da-n hɩɩn wɩrɛ tɔɔnɩ dɩko kho paarra, dɩ a yɩrɛ le kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ na tɔnɩ he kɩ̃kɩɩna'.
40022012	Dɩ a buleele: Ɩ̃ kuun, mɔ̃ fɩ fʋ sa lõ kɩɛr, sɩ fa to he kɩ̃kɩɩna'; dɩ kuunile pɩr pɔbɩ.
40022013	Le fãgadaarɩle so thɔ̃darara: Nɩ fʋɔnɛɛ a le nɛɛ na nyɛ̃ɛ a dɔna faa jɩɛra dabirə paar, ka wa bɩnɩ wa-n yɩrna nyɩma.
40022014	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ wɩ wenɩ wɩ jɔrɛ kpɛ, sɩ wɩrɛ wɩ phiirni wa kpɛra'.
40022015	Le jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ jal dɩ wa-n gʋʋr kha, mɔ̃ wa fʋnɩ sɩ na nɔ Jeju thɩmɩɩraakɛ a na mɩɩnɩ.
40022016	Dɩ wɩ thʋɔn ɔɔ pa awɩ kpãkpãadarasɔ na Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ too, dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa ayɩ: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sobɔ tibil fɩ do, dɩ fɩ-n dɩɩrɛ dakha Thãgbaa hʋ na sobɔr sɩ fa-n ma tibilə', gɩdonɩ fa-n hɩɩn tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa';
40022017	dɩ gɛr gɩ sɔ sar mɔ̃ fɩ yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ ha. Gɩ teere kha dɩ sa lɩmɩ Sejaar lãpho yaa, ga tee kha ga.
40022018	Sɩ gɩdonɩ Jeju jɩrɛ awɩ bɩ̃ kpal thɩmɩɩ, a birse wer: Nɛr bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n fifilə mi?
40022019	Nɩ nɛ mar warɩkɛra nɩ-n gbanɩ dɩ nɩ lɩmɩ lãphora. Dɩ wɩ gba war birera a pɔna.
40022020	Dɩ a bule wer: Amɛ ha ʋrɛ fotoraakɛ, dɩ amɛɛ khere ha gɩrɛ?
40022021	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Sejaar gɩ. Dɩ mɛ̃ a so war ayɩ: Nɩ 'laanɛ Sejaarra gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Sejaarɩda, a 'laanɛ Thãgbara gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaada.
40022022	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɛr thɩmɩɩraale wɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ, dɩ wɩ gba faa sa jal kɔ̃.
40022023	Ga wi bɩɛlɩlera Sadʋsɛ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala', pɔr Jejura a bulee bulele thakɛ ayɩ:
40022024	Dɩɩrdaar, Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sor ayɩ: “A tibil hana khɛr sa khi sɩ bɩsaan na hala', ɔɔ õkuun n gba khikhɛrʋʋlera a hɛ a kɔna bɩsana wɩ do ɔɔ õkuuni məl.”
40022025	Sɩɩ do õkona makonyɔ wɛ a kɔɔ hale asɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ cacadaar kɔɔ her khɛr a khi, sɩ gɩdonɩ bɩsaan na hala' dɩɩ do ɔɔ õkuunna a faa khɛrɩle mɛ̃.
40022026	Thalera gɩ kɔɔ ha na balanyɔdaar, agɩpɩ na balãtherdaar, a jalna thalera waa a ba dana makonyɔdaar.
40022027	A wele pɩ fɛʋ na pɩ, khɛr dakha khire.
40022028	Dɩ gɛr gɩ, ado khe na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera, ʋmɔ̃ wɛr makonyɔra na hɩna khɛrɩlera dɩphã gɩrɛ, gɩdonɩ wɛr fɛʋra kɔɔ hɩɛ.
40022029	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Jaa, nɩ buure waa fĩi koe, gɩdonɩ na jɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ na Thãgbaa fãga ga, gɛr gɩ.
40022030	Gɩdonɩ ado khe na ɩɩr na the khirera, kona na he khɛra bã, dɩ khɛra dakha na he kona bã, sɩ wa hʋrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛ hanɩle Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
40022031	Sɩ ado khee ɩɩr gɩ, na kɔɔ yɩɛ le Thãgbaa sɛbɛra gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgba so narnaa?
40022032	Mee ayɩ: “Ɩnɛr dʋɔn Abɩrahamɩ Thãgba, na Ɩjakɩɩ Thãgba, na Jakɔbɩɩ Thãgba.” Thãgba na do khee Thãgba ga, sɩ wɩrɛ hananɩ yiree Thãgba a do.
40022033	Dɩ tibil jɔɔkɛ hande dɩ wa-n pɛ nũu, nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɛr Jejuu dɩɩrra.
40022034	Mɔ̃ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ, a cʋʋrɛ wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala', dɩ wa yɩ nʋɔ bã, wɩ kpar kha a pɔ.
40022035	Dɩ tibil bɩɛl wɛrraakɛ dɔnɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar ɩɩrnanaa bule ʋrɛ wo, da-n fifiləə a hɩɩn ayɩ:
40022036	Dɩɩrdaar, ʋmɔ̃ dɔrakɛ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ a jɔ jɔfʋsɔ fɛʋ?
40022037	Dɩ Jeju birsee: “Dɔ fa-n na Kɔ̃tɩn afɩ Thãgba na afɩ bɩ̃ fɛʋ, na afɩ ha fɛʋ, na afɩ kpɩɛr fɛʋ.”
40022038	Ɔr dʋɔn cacadaa, kɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ jɔfʋsɔ fɛʋ.
40022039	Dɩ yɛ kɛ balanyɔdaa wo kɛ n hʋɔnɛɛnɩ: “Dɔ fa-n na afɩ 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃kɛ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara.”
40022040	Jɔfʋ yenyɔraakɛ jɔfʋ fɛʋ na Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ so jəəro yʋʋ fɛʋ.
40022041	Mɔ̃ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kpanɩ kha a jɛ, Jeju bule wer thɩ̃ɛ ayɩ:
40022042	Anye nɩ-n kpɩɛrna Kirisiti? Amɛɛ bikuun a do? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun gɩ.
40022043	Dɩ Jeju so war: Dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ Thu Phuu cʋʋ Davɩdɩ da-n wɩɩ Kɔ̃tɩn, ɔbɔɔkɛ a sonɩ ayɩ:
40022044	“Thãgba sor ɩ̃ Kɔ̃tɩna ayɩ: Tɔɔ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra, phaphapha ɩ̃ cʋʋ afɩ lãlaardara wɩ do afɩ nɛ jəəda.”
40022045	Dɩ ado Davɩdɩ n wɩɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn thale, mɔ̃ a na fʋ sɩ na do ɔɔ bikuun?
40022046	Dɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na puno na deeraa ga. Dɩ a fʋna ga wiile tibil na-n 'la dɩ bulee thɩ̃ɛ bã.
40023001	Le Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩna tibil jɔɔle nakha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara ayɩwɔɔ:
40023002	Jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ fien gba Mʋɩjɩɩ too pa dɩ wa-n mɩɛ tɩbɩla jɔfʋ kɩrʋ.
40023003	Gɛr gɩ, nɩ hɩnɛ a na cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ-n so narnɩ, sɩ na-n cʋʋ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n cʋʋna', gɩdonɩ nʋɔ wɩ-n sona sɩ wa-n cʋa'.
40023004	Wɩ-n lire heendaasɔɔkɛ dɩbarɔnɩ dɩ wɩ heen tɩbɩla, sɩ awɩ thɛthɛ na-n ƴaal wɩ tharna awɩ nyɛ̃ fɩɩʋraka'.
40023005	Wɩ-n cʋʋrɛ awɩ thɩ̃ fɛʋ tɩbɩla na-n yɛ wɩ. Gɛr n dɔ nɔɔ dɩ wɩ cʋʋ awɩ lo kɛra dɩɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃, dɩ wɩ cʋʋ dakha awɩ kẽkẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃ nɔsɔ dɩɩ gbaan jʋɔljʋɔl.
40023006	Wɩ-n nar ƴɛ kʋʋl too paar dɩko kho paar na ƴɛ kʋʋl too paar awɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔsɔra.
40023007	Wɩ-n nar tɩbɩla na-n fʋɔrɛ wɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋ a na wɛna wɩ dakha dɩɩrdara.
40023008	Sɩ ne wer, na-n do tɩbɩla na-n we nɩ dɩɩrdara ga, gɩdonɩ bɩɛl dɩbara 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ dʋɔn anɩ Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ omɩna nɩ do.
40023009	Dɩ na-n we tibil thɩɩra anɩ tha', gɩdonɩ bɩɛl dɩbara haanle kɛ dɔnɩ anɩ Thɩ, ʋrɛɛkɛ hanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ.
40023010	Na-n do wa-n we nɩ kɔ̃tɩna ga, gɩdonɩ bɩɛl dɩbara haanle kɛ dɔnɩ anɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃, Kirisiti gɩ.
40023011	Sɩ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩn anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a jɔ, ɔr na ka na do anɩ thɔ̃daar.
40023012	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n kanɩ ire wa wuruure, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n wuroni dɩbara, ɔr wa ɩɩr.
40023013	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n khaanɛ ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ hʋ tɩbɩlala, nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛɛkɛ yɛnɩ na-n lõa', dɩ wɩrɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ wɩ lõ wo na-n sɩ war wɩ lona ga.
40023014	[Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n phʋʋnɛ khikhɛra sɩɩ do fɩɩlɛ nɩ-n bɩɛlna Thãgba dɩ nɩ pʋɔrna ƴɛrr tɩbɩla na-n yɛ nɩ dɩphã. Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ so kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na heen nɩ na khɩɩr na ka.]
40023015	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n pɩrɛ paar fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ na lanyʋɔnna tɩɩ bɩɛlla nɩ cʋgʋʋ a fe a hɔ Juifi. Dɩ ado a debi pɩ, dɩɩ do nɩ ka cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ do bu paarɩ bɩsã dɩ jɔ nɩ balanyɔ.
40023016	Ga puu narɛ nɛr thɔthɔɔda yarasɔɔkɛ n sɔnɩ dɩ nɩ yɩ: Ado tibil ʋlfɛna Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔr aa, ga do puure ga. Sɩ ado ntɛ ʋlfɛna dɛɛkɛ hanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔr, a toorore.
40023017	Nɛr də̃bələ na yarasɔ, ʋmɔ̃ ka do dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ a jɔ? Dɛ gɩ yaa, Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɩkɛ n cʋɛnɩ dɛ dɩɩ do thɩ̃ phuu gɩ?
40023018	Nɩ sor wo ayɩ: Ado tibil ʋlfɛna bonɩ ji paar aa, ga do puure ga. Sɩ ado ntɛ ʋlfɛna bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɛɛnɛnɩ bonɩ ji paar, a toorore.
40023019	Yara ha nɩ bã, ʋmɔ̃ ka do dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ a jɔ? Bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛ gɩ yaa, bonɩ ji paarɩkɛ n cʋɛnɩ bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ do daphuu gɩ?
40023020	Ʋrɛ ʋlfɛnanɩ bonɩ ji paar, bonɩ ji paarra a ʋlfɛna na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ harɔnɩ.
40023021	Dɩ ʋrɛ ʋlfɛnanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔr, Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrra a ʋlfɛna na ʋrɛ n cɔrɔnɩ.
40023022	Dɩ ʋrɛ ʋlfɛnanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, Thãgbaa fãga too pa a ʋlfɛna na ʋrɛɛkɛ n tɔɔrɔnɩ.
40023023	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n tire bɩɛl yʋɔr anɩ bi fara na anɩ thɩ̃ phulosɔraakɛ fɛʋ dʋɔnnɩ bii, sɩ dɩ nɩ ka hɛbɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩɩnaakɛ jɔfʋra a faa, kɛ dɔnɩ fɩl sarʋ, na bɔ jɩɩr, na sobɔ cʋʋrɛ. Sɩ gɛr ka do thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ teenanɩ nɩ cʋʋ, sɩ ga do wɩ yɩ nɩ hɛba gelela ga.
40023024	Nɛr thɔthɔɔda yarasɔ, nɩ-n tɛr cĩcinə a na faa, sɩ dɩ na-n dɩɩ nyɔɔmɛ.
40023025	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n cɔcɔɔrɛ thɩ̃ yɔdaa na dɩko khodaa khiru, sɩɩ do bɩnɔ nɩ ka hire na thɩ̃ tagɩrɩ kpɩɛrɛ na dɩbara fʋ thʋnɔnɛ.
40023026	Fɛr jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaarɩkɛ yaarɛnɩ, dɔ fɩ cɔcɔɔ thɩ̃ yɔdaa na dɩko khodaa bɩnɛ ɓo, ɔmɛ̃ khiru na hɩrɛ.
40023027	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ hʋrɛ kaakɛ wɩ calnɩ mɩlɛ, dɩɩ do jɩɛra wer gɩ bɔrɛ hɩɩnɛna, sɩ dɩɩ do bɩnɔ khi khubo he le na thɩ̃ bise caar fɛʋ.
40023028	Mɛ̃ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ ha; jɩɛra wer, nɩ-n hʋrɛ tɩɩ sara tɩbɩlala, sɩ bɩnɔ, bɩnɛ yenyɔ fɩlɛ he le na sopugo.
40023029	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n mɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ ka, dɩ na-n gbɛbɩ tɩɩ sarasɔɔ ka gɩ bʋɔnɔ,
40023030	sɩ dɩ na-n so dɩ nɩ yɩ aa: Ado sɛr kɔɔ haanle asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ bɔɔle, sa kɔɔ tu awɩdaale a na deer Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔlee tɔmã'.
40023031	Thakɛrakɛ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n nɩnanɛ, dɩ nɛr dʋɔn wɩrɛ kɔɔ kʋrɛnɩ Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔlee bɩsãsɔ.
40023032	Dɩ gɛr gɩ nɩ yɩra pɩɩrɛ anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ thɔ̃ puurə mɛ̃.
40023033	Nɛr siisɔ, sikori bisɔ, mɔ̃ na cʋʋ sɩ na the so heenenaakɛ na jalana nɩnɩ bu paar dɔɔra?
40023034	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma thɔna nar Thãgbaa bobonasɔ, na tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔ, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ, dɩ na kʋʋrɛ ɩkhasɔ, na gba ɩkhasɔ na kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra, na ciil ɩkhasɔ na khasa awɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔsɔra, na kpoo warɛ dɩɩ wo dɩɩra;
40023035	dɩ mɛ̃ sor na heen nɩ dɩphã dɩ pa 'leedaraa tɔmɩnaakɛ fɛʋ, kɛ kɔɔ deerenɩ thɩɩraakɛ dɩɩ fʋna Abɛl tɩɩ sarʋʋ tɔmɩ̃ a jalna waa a ba dana Barasɩɩ bikuun Jakarɩɩ tɔmɩ̃, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ nɩ kɔɔ kʋnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔr na bonɩ ji pa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
40023036	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, gele fɛʋ na heene nĩdaraakɛ sor.
40023037	Pha Jerujalɛm, Jerujalɛm, fɛrkɛ n kʋrɛnɩ Thãgbaa bobona, dɩ fa-n dʋʋrna wɩrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ thɔ̃ farnɩ bokana, balamɔ̃ balamɔ̃ mɩ kɔɔ ƴaal ɩ̃ gbɛbɩra afɩ too mɔ̃kɛ yɔl nɩɩ n gbɛbɩnɩ ɔɔ bisɔ dɩ thiro gbɛla, sɩ na kɔɔ tuə'.
40023038	Dɩ nɩ hɩnɛ dɩphã, wa faa narɛ anɩ cɔra dɩ ga do cɔ kpoloo,
40023039	gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ ayɩ: A fʋna nɛnɛ̃kɛ na yɩ mɩ bã, phaphapha gɩ dana bɔɔkɛ na sonɩ nayɩ: “Ʋrɛ n ɩnanɩ na Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i hɩna khɩɩrɛ.”
40024001	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju thenɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna da-n gba hʋɛ, ɔɔ kpãkpãadara tɔr pʋɔraa a nɩɩraa mɔ̃ wɩ mɩnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle.
40024002	Sɩ a birse wer ayɩ: Nɩ yɩrɛ gelesɔra fɛʋaa? Sobɔr mɩ so nar, na yɩ kɩɛr boka bɩɛl dɩ na bir na sɩ na dɛ̃ɛ ʋ̃ bokara ƴũ bã, fɛʋ na derre.
40024003	Mɔ̃ Jeju toonɩ gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra, kpãkpãadara kɔɔ pɔr a bulee hɛllɩ: So sar bɔɔkɛ gelela na danɩ, na gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ afɩ bir ɩ̃ bɔ jẽ, na thɩɩkɛɛ pɩ bɔda.
40024004	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, na-n do tibil n fɩɩl na';
40024005	gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla bərəəm na gbaar ɩ̃ i na ɩna wa-n so wɩ yɩ, ɩnɛr dʋɔn Kirisitira; dɩ mɛ̃ wa fɩɩl tɩbɩla jɔɔ.
40024006	Na nɩɛrɛ ko thɩmɩasɔ, na nɩɛrɛ wa-n mɩɩ aa, kʋʋr na hale. A nɩ jɩ, na-n do maar n fʋ na', gɩdonɩ dɔ gele n kɔɔ dã, sɩ ga do gɛr na dʋɔn thɩ pɩ paar pa'.
40024007	Ʋ ca na ɩɩrɛ a na-n kena ʋ̃ ca, ʋ̃ fãgadaarɩ dɩ bɩɛl n ɩɩr a na-n kena ʋ̃ fãgadaarɩ dɩ kpɩɩ. Dɩ kɔmɛ kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na thɩ jɩɩnsɔ na hale paar dɩɩdɩɩsɔ dakha.
40024008	Sɩ gele fɛʋ bɔ gaarɛɛ fʋ pa gɩ dɩbara.
40024009	Ɔbɔɔle tɩbɩla na fʋlɛ nɩ a na gaar nɩ bʋɔ dɩ wa kʋʋr nɛr, dɩ tibil caar fɛʋ na-n laar nɛr, gɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ.
40024010	Dɩ mɛ̃ ga do nɛ baradaa tibil jɔjʋɔra, dɩ tɩbɩla na-n liire khasɔ wa-n laarna khasɔ dɩɩdɩɩ.
40024011	Sõso bobonasɔ na ɩɩrɛ wa-n fɩɩl tɩbɩla bərəəm.
40024012	Dɩ gɩdonɩ puure na jɔrɛ ga-n pɛr, ga dor nɔɔ dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ na hana naʋ bã.
40024013	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na yɩranɩ na dana khu paar, ɔr na 'lɛ taarɛ.
40024014	Sɩ dɔ wɩ mɩɩ ƴũ fãgadaar tutugo bɔ thɩmɩɩkɛ thɩɩraakɛ koo, gɩ mɩɩ ha pɛdaa tibil caarra fɛʋ. Liir dɩphã na dɔ thɩ pɩ paar mɛ̃.
40024015	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ ɔbɔɔkɛ na yɩnɩ thɩ̃ thuurnəəkɛ na kʋɛanɩ thɩ̃ɛ, kɛ Thãgbaa bobon Danɩɛl kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ dɩ ga ha pa phuurə (dɔ ʋrɛ n hɩnɛnɩ sɛbɛɛkɛ n dʋ gar bʋrɛ),
40024016	le wɩrɛ hanɩ Jude n fuo ca jala gɔ̃gʋɔna,
40024017	dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hanɩ nãsʋrɔ a na-n gbũ cʋɔrɔ a gba thɩ̃a',
40024018	dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ dakha na hanɩ lɔɔ, a na-n kɛr bir a gba ɔɔ kẽkẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bã.
40024019	Ga wisɔɔle, ga puurore khɛ pɛmɛdarara na wɩrɛ n mamanɩ bibɔrɔsɔ.
40024020	Na-n bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba dɩ anɩ fuu bɔɔle na-n do yʋʋrɔa', agɩbo hɩɩr wirə'.
40024021	Gɩdonɩ bɔ gaarɛɛle na kɔ̃tɩnɛ na ka, bɔ gaar caa thale na kɔɔ hale kpɩɩrakɛ a fʋna bɔɔkɛ Thãgba tini thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ ba dana nɛnɛ̃ka', dɩ ga bir na halerakɛ kpɩɩ bã.
40024022	Ado wiresɔɔle na kɔɔ tɔ a gburoə', tibil bɩɛllakɛ na mar na ta ga, sɩ wɩrɛ Thãgba phiirni dɔ kɩrʋ da tɔ wiresɔɔle dɩ ga gburo.
40024023	Dɩ dabɔɔle ado tibil na so nar nayɩ: Nɩ hɩnɛ, Kirisiti har kɩɛr agɩbo a ha pal, na-n pɛr haara'.
40024024	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n sõsonenɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ, Kirisiti ha nɩ, agɩbo bobona ha nɩ, na ɩɩrɛ wa-n nɩna tɩbɩla nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔ, wa-n fɩɩlnanakɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ phiirni, adora hʋɛ hale.
40024025	Dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ mãa dɩ ma-n so nar gɩrɛ.
40024026	Ado wɩ so nar ayɩ: Bəənnə a ha, na-n jalaa dɛ, agɩbo: Du bɩnɔ a ha, na-n pɛ gɩ haara'.
40024027	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ thãgba n lenɩ dɔɔ wi phã paar dɩɩ carbara a ka a dã wi lõ paar, thale mɛr tibili Bikuuni bir ɩ̃ na ha.
40024028	Kãkɛ thɩ̃ khire hanɩ, le dũusɔ na caan kha.
40024029	Ga bɔɔlera, a bɔ gaarɛ ka na pɩ, dapaara wire na birəre, por dakha na hɩrɛ bã, ƴepələ̃be na ther thãgbara ƴũ ga-n jɛ thɩɩra, dɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ fãgaakɛ hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ ga gbugbuyore.
40024030	Liiir dɩphã wa yɩ mɛr tibili Bikuuni jẽ dɩ ga yɩr thãgbara ƴũ, dɩ tibil caar fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ na-n bɩrɛ, gɩdonɩ wa yɩrɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun ma-n ɩ̃ na ndɔlɔ̃pana na fãga, na carbararɛ jɔɔ.
40024031	Dɩ ma thʋɔn ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ wa-n ʋ̃ tutuu kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, sɩ wɩ kpa wɩrɛ Thãgba phiirni, kɛ hanɩ kɩrrɔ, na gananɔ, na gɛla yenyɔra fɛʋ, wɩ jɛ pa bɩɛl gɩ fʋna ka thãgbara ƴũ khuni gɩ dana ʋ̃ khu pa.
40024032	Sɩ nɩ dɔ sokpaa thɩr khonanɛdara n dɩɩr nɩ thɩ̃ɛ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ yɩnɩ ɔɔ jɛ̃sɔ dɩɩ ɓol a na thɔɔ fa ƴolo, nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ ubulo n wɩla.
40024033	Mɛ̃ gɩ, nɛrɛ dakha, ado na yɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔle fɛʋ, nɩ jɛ dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuuni ɩ̃ bɔ n daan, dɩ mɩ har lõfonɔɔ.
40024034	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, nĩdaraakɛ na khiir koo, sɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ fɛʋ n dã ga.
40024035	Thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩ na phor na ka, sɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔ na pho na ka kpɩɩraka'.
40024036	Sɩ ado wi jɩɩrra gɩ, na bɔɔkɛ ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ na danɩ, tibil bɩɛllakɛ na jɩ ga, thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔrakɛ le Thãgbaa dʋɔ wa ja', Bikuunnakɛ na ja', sɩ Thɩrɛ dɩbara jɩɛn gɩ.
40024037	Mɔ̃kɛ thɩ̃ɛ kɔɔ hanɩ Noee bɔɔ, mɛna ga ha tibili Bikuuni ɩna.
40024038	Gɩdonɩ wiresɔɔkɛ kɔɔ kanɩ, sɩ thɩ̃ kʋɛ nyʋɔnɩle na-n kpaan, tɩbɩla n kɔɔ khor dɩkɔ, dɩ wa-n yɔna, dɩ wa-n hena kha, dɩ wa-n 'laana awɩ bisɔ herra, phaphapha dɩɩ ba dana wireekɛ Noe kɔɔ lonɩ batora.
40024039	Sɩrakɛ wa-n kɔɔ dɛna dɩkha ga, foo dɩ nyʋɔn phã a gbʋma wɩ dɩ wɩ khiir fɛʋ. Ɔmɛna ga ha tibili Bikuuni ɩna.
40024040	Ga wiile kona yenyɔɔkɛ na hanɩ lɛ bɩɛlla, Thãgba na gbaar bɩɛl sɩ na faa bɩɛl.
40024041	Dɩ khɛra yenyɔɔkɛ na hanɩ kha jʋ nã paar, Thãgba na gbaar bɩɛl sɩ na faa bɩɛl.
40024042	Gɛr gɩ a nɩ jɩ na-n jʋrɛ, gɩdonɩ na jɩ wireekɛ anɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na ɩna'.
40024043	Nɩ jɩɛ jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ bɔɔbɔɔ, ado cɔdaar kuun jɩrɛ bɔ dɔɔkɛ yu na pɔnɩ ɔɔ cɔ dɩtɩnɔ, a na-n bɛrɛ a na sɩɩraa a lʋʋn cʋɔrɔa'.
40024044	Gɛr gɩ nɛrɛ dakha, nɩ gbɛbɩrɛ pɛ, gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na bire na ɩ̃ bɔɔkɛ na kpɩɛrna mɩna'.
40024045	Ʋmɔ̃ dɔ sobɔ cʋʋ thɔ̃daar, kɛ kpɛsɛnɛnɩ, dɩ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na pɛr a na-n hɩnɛ ɔɔ cɔdara a na hana wɩ dɩkɔ bɔɔkɛ gɩ teenɩ kha?
40024046	Ga dar thɔ̃daar ca olela, ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na-n danɩ a yɩɩ a na-n cʋʋ mɛ̃.
40024047	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na jɩɛ cʋgʋʋ a do ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔ fɛʋʋ hɩɩndaar.
40024048	Sɩ ado thɔ̃daar puu gɩ, a na sor ɔɔbarara nayɩ: Ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩna n pʋɔrɛ ɩɩnna kpɛ;
40024049	dɩ ado a mar da-n bɩɩr ɔɔ 'walãkhasɔɔkɛ a-n donanɩ kha thɔma, dɩ khona da-n yɔna nakha ta 'laardara.
40024050	Thɔ̃daar ca olee kɔ̃tɩ̃ na phurore, dawiikɛ aa-n pɩɛrʋʋna', na bɔɔraakɛ aa kpɩɛrnana';
40024051	dɩ a na cɩɩrɛ yɩra yɩra, sɩ na gbaa na pɛ wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, paarɩkɛra wa bɩnɩ wa-n yɩrna nyɩma.
40025001	Ga bɔɔle, ƴũ fãgadaarɩ dɩ ga hʋrɛ khɛ biirə yʋɔrɩkɛ na jɛnɩ kuun pa', kɛ kɔɔ gbaannɩ awɩ lãphãsɔ a jal wɩ caan khɛrɩ ko.
40025002	Yemɔɩ wɛrra dor də̃bələ, sɩ yemɔɩ do khɛ bi kpɛsɛsɔ.
40025003	Də̃bələ gbaar awɩ lãphãsɔ sɩ wa kɔɔ gba niinə',
40025004	sɩ khɛ bi kpɛsɛsɔɔle gbaar awɩ lãphãsɔ a gbana niin na nĩ pɛdaa a fʋrɔ.
40025005	Mɔ̃ khɛrɩ ko n pʋɔrnɩ pʋɔrra, dayuur fʋlɛ wɛr fɛʋ dɩ wa-n daar.
40025006	A dɩɩ nɩrɔ hulẽbire ther aa: Nɩ yɛ khɛrɩ ko, nɩ thɛ na caanɛɛ.
40025007	Dɩ khɛ biirəəle fɛʋ pal ɩɩr a ma dɩ wa-n gbɛbɩ awɩ lãphãsɔ.
40025008	Dɩ khɛ bi də̃bələəle so khɛ bi kpɛsɛsɔra ayɩ: Nɩ pɛ sar anɩ ninə gbe, gɩdonɩ asɩ lãphãsɔ n khiire.
40025009	Dɩ khɛ bi kpɛsɛsɔɔle birse wi: Ǝ̃'ə̃, gɩdonɩ ga dã sɩ kha na nɛrɛa', nɩ jala wɩrɛraakɛ n dolonenɩ a thɛ anɩda.
40025010	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ jalnɩ wɩ the, dɩɩ do khɛrɩ ko daan, dɩ khɛ bi wele kɔɔ gbɛbɩrɛnɩ pɩ, cʋrrɛ kha a lõ he fɛtɩ cʋgʋʋ, sɩ dɩ loo khaan.
40025011	Ga too gbe dɩ wa khɛ bisɔɔle pɔ dakha wer dɩ wa-n so: Kɔ̃tɩn, Kɔ̃tɩn, khɛra sɩ loo.
40025012	Dɩ birse wi: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ma jɩ na'.
40025013	Gɛr gɩ a nɩ jɩ na-n jʋrɛ, gɩdonɩ na jɩ wire dɩ bɔɔ ga.
40025014	Ga hʋrɛ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ kɔɔ ƴaalɛnɩ a kpaar, a we ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔ, a pɛ war ɔɔ lẽle thɩ̃sɔ wa-n hɩnɛ.
40025015	Dɩ a har bɩɛl war bɔrɔ yemɔɩ, a ha bɩɛl war bɔrɔ yenyɔ, sa ha balãtherdaar war bɔrɔ bɩɛl. A ha wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl mɔ̃ awɩ puno hanɩ, sa gba jal kpaar paar.
40025016	Dapaara ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ war bɔrɔ yemɔɩ gbaar jalna da-n ƴabɩna, a 'lɛ yemɔɩ a dɛɛnɔ wo.
40025017	Mɛ̃ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ war bɔrɔ yenyɔ 'lɛ yenyɔ wo a dɛɛnɔ.
40025018	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ war bɔrɔ bɩɛl dɩbara, a jaal a kpe koru a puu le ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ war faa.
40025019	A gɩ ɩ̃ a pʋɔr thɔ̃daraalee kɔ̃tɩna bire ɩ̃, a we wɩ wɩ thera war ɩnɩ-n hɩɩn.
40025020	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ war bɔrɔ yemɔɩɩle tɔr dã na dɛɛnɛ yemɔɩɩkɛ a 'lɛnɩ a so: Kɔ̃tɩn, fɩ kɔɔ pɛ marɛ war bɔrɔ yemɔɩ. Yɛ yemɔɩ phaa mɩ birni 'lɛ a dɛɛnɔ.
40025021	Dɩ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ sʋʋraa: Gɩ bɔrɛ kpɛ, thɔ̃daar bʋɔ ha fɩ na sobɔ cʋʋdaar. Fɩ kɔɔ dor sobɔ cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ fɩɩʋra, nɛnɛ̃ ma pɛ farɛ dɩ fa do hɩɩndaar thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔra. Lona daʋraakɛ dɔnɩ afɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩda.
40025022	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ war bɔrɔ yenyɔ tɔ dã a so: Kɔ̃tɩn fɩ kɔɔ pɛ marɛ war bɔrɔ yenyɔ, yɛ kɛ yenyɔ phaa mɩ birni 'lɛ a dɛɛnɔ wo.
40025023	Dɩ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ sʋʋraa: Gɩ bɔrɛ kpɛ, thɔ̃daar bʋɔ ha fɩ na sobɔ cʋʋdaar. Fɩ kɔɔ dor sobɔ cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ fɩɩʋra, nɛnɛ̃ ma pɛ farɛ dɩ fa do hɩɩndaar thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔra. Lona daʋraakɛ dɔnɩ afɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩda.
40025024	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ war bɔrɔ bɩɛl dɩbara tɔr dã dakha a so: Kɔ̃tɩn, mɩ jɩrɛ fɛr dɔ tibilikɛ afɩda khɩɩrnɩ, dɩ fa-n kha jɔ kãkɛ fa diirnə', dɩ fa-n kha kãkɛ fa kɔɔ jalnɩ woa'.
40025025	Gɛr gɩ maar kɔɔ fʋ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ gba afɩ bɔrɔ bɩɛlla a puu thɩɩra. Gɩkɛ gba, gɛr dɔ afɩda.
40025026	Dɩ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ birsee ayɩ: Fɛr thɔ̃daar puu na khãkhal, fɩ kɔɔ jɩrɛ dɩ mɛr dɔ ʋrɛ n khanɩ kãkɛ ma kɔɔ diirnə', dɩ ma-n kha dakha kãkɛ ma kɔɔ jalnɩ thɩ̃a',
40025027	dɩ gɩ kɔɔ teenanɛna wɩ yɛ fɩ gbaar ɩ̃ war a 'laa kãkɛ ma 'lɛrɔnɩ khor. A mɩ kɛrrɛ bir ɩ̃, ɩ̃ gba ɩ̃da na khor.
40025028	Dɩ gɛr gɩ, nɩ taaraa bɔrɔ bɩɛlɩle a hananɩ, a hana ʋrɛ hananɩ bɔrɔ yʋɔrɩle.
40025029	Gɩdonɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ hananɩ thɩ̃ɛ, wa bire na haa na dɛbɩrɔ wo, dɩ na hana gɩ dɩ ga jɩɩ jɔr. Sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na hananɩ thɩ̃a', wa tiirəərerakɛ phubi gɩrɛ a hananɩ.
40025030	Sɩ olela na dɔnɩ bɔ taa thɔ̃daara', nɩ dɔnaa jɩɛra dabirə paar faa, kãkɛ wa bɩnɩ wa-n yɩrna nyɩma.
40025031	Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun na-n ɩnɩ na ɩ̃ i dʋbɩ nakha ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ fɛʋ, ma toore ɩ̃ i dʋbɩ fãga too para.
40025032	Dɩ le wa kpa tibil caar fɛʋ na jɛ ɩ̃ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ ma leere wɛ na wɛ, mɔ̃kɛ bana khedaar n leenɩ banaa na bɔ.
40025033	Dɩ ma pɛr banaa ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra, sɩ ɩ̃ pɛ bɔ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɩlana.
40025034	Le mɛr fãgadaar na so wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra ɩ̃ yɩ: Nɩ ɩna nɛrkɛ ɩ̃ Thɩ bɔnanɩ, a gba fãgadaar dɩɩkɛ wɩ kɔɔ maanɩ gbɛbɩ nar kɛkɛkɛ thɩɩkɛ ti bɔɔ a hɩna.
40025035	Gɩdonɩ kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋ mɛr dɩ nɩ kɔɔ ha mɩ dɩkor; yɔlkhaa kɔɔ fʋ mɛr dɩ nɩ kɔɔ ha mɩ nyʋɔn; mɩ kɔɔ dor kpakpal dɩ nɩ kɔɔ tee mɩ;
40025036	mɩ kɔɔ hananɛ sãɓɔlɔ̃ dɩ nɩ kɔɔ saa mɩ kɩ̃kɩɩn; gɩ-n kɔɔ kho mer dɩ nɩ kɔɔ pɔ a yɩ mɩ; mɩ kɔɔ har khaɩra dɩ nɩ kɔɔ pɔ a yɩ mɩ.
40025037	Le tɩɩ sarasɔ na birse mi nayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ sɩ kɔɔ yɩ fɩ na kɔmɛr a ha fɩ dɩkor, dɩ yɔlkhaa kɔɔ fʋ fɩ dɩ sɩ kɔɔ ha fɩ nyʋɔn?
40025038	Ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ sɩ kɔɔ yɩ fɩ dɩ fɩ kɔɔ do kpakpal dɩ sɩ kɔɔ tee fɩ, agɩbo na sãɓɔlɔ̃ dɩ sɩ kɔɔ ha fɩ kɩ̃kɩɩn?
40025039	Ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ sɩ kɔɔ yɩ fɩ dɩ ga-n kho fɩ, agɩbo dɩ fɩ kɔɔ ha khaɩra dɩ sɩ kɔɔ pɔ a yɩ fɩ?
40025040	Dɩ mɛr fãgadaar na birse wer nayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ nɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ ɩ̃ omi bu fɩɩʋra, mɛrra nɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ.
40025041	Agɩpɩ, ma sor wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɩlana: Nɩ hala mɩ jala ƴɔɔ, nɛrkɛ so kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ heennɩ, nɩ jala lona khorr dɔɔraakɛ wɩ gbɛbɩnɩ thɩɩn Satana, na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔra.
40025042	Gɩdonɩ kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋ mɛr sɩ na kɔɔ ha mɩ dɩkora'; yɔlkhaa kɔɔ fʋ mɛr sɩ na kɔɔ ha mɩ nyʋɔna';
40025043	mɩ kɔɔ dor kpakpal sɩ na kɔɔ tee ma'; mɩ kɔɔ hananɛ sãɓɔlɔ̃ sɩ na kɔɔ ha mɩ kɩ̃kɩɩna'; gɩ-n kɔɔ kho mer dɩ mɩ kɔɔ har dakha khaɩra, sɩ na kɔɔ pɔ a yɩ ma'.
40025044	Dɩ le wa birse mi dakha nayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ sɩ kɔɔ yɩ fɩ na kɔmɛr na yɔlkhaa, agɩbo dɩ fɩ kɔɔ do kpakpal, agɩbo dɩ fɩ kɔɔ hana sãɓɔlɔ̃, dɩ ga-n kho fɩ dakha, agɩbo wo dɩ fɩ ha khaɩra dɩ sa kɔɔ cʋʋ fɩ bɔa'.
40025045	Dɩ le ma birse wi nayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ ɩ̃ omi bu fɩɩʋra ga, mɛrra na kɔɔ cʋa'.
40025046	Dɩ wɛr, wa jaal khorr so 'lɛ paar, sɩ tɩɩ sara n 'lɛ yire khorr.
40026001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju mɩɩnɩ thɩmɩaakɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ pɩ, a sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ:
40026002	Nɩ jɩrɛ wire yenyɔ sɛ sɩ Pakɩ n dã, dɩ wa fʋrɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun na kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
40026003	Ɔbɔɔlera bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na tɩbɩlaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kpa kha a jɛ Kaɩfɩ gbõdaarɩ gbayara,
40026004	a gʋʋr kha mɔ̃ wa cʋʋnɩ sɩ na fʋ Jeju na fɩɩlɛ a na kʋ.
40026005	Sɩ wɩ-n sor aa, wa-n do gɩ do bɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla hanɩ fɛtɩ cʋʋrɔ kĩkĩkə̃', a mɛ̃ gaa ga hor khʋ̃ɛ na har tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
40026006	Mɔ̃ Jeju hanɩ Betanɩ Sɩmɔ̃ gbuuluu cɔ,
40026007	khɛ bɩɛl pʋɔraarɛ le a fʋrɔ laaso ja bʋlabir, kɛ hananɩ latɩkolo niinikɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ ka. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju hanɩ dɩko kho paar, khɛrɩle lʋʋn le a deer latɩkolookɛ Jejuu yʋra.
40026008	Mɔ̃ kpãkpãadara yɩɛnɩ thale, nĩkhii fʋlɛ wɛr dɩ wɩ so ayɩ: Anyee thɩ̃ kʋɛ ca ha gɩrɛ thakɛ?
40026009	Ga do wa kɔɔ dolone latɩkolo niinile gɩ khɩɩr, wɩ gba warɩle wɩ ha bɔdara gaa?
40026010	Dɩ Jeju jɩrɛ a so war: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n pɛ khɛrɩkɛ nɩwɛ? Thɔ̃ bʋɔ a cʋʋ mar waa gel.
40026011	Sɩ ado bɔdara wɛ, wɩ har anɩ pa wire fɛʋ, sɩ ado mɛr gɩ, ga do wire fɛʋ na hana ma'.
40026012	Sɩ mɔ̃ a deernɩ latɩkolo niinikɛ ɩ̃ tomɩra, a gbɛbɩ mɛr mɔ̃ wa dʋ mɩnɩ.
40026013	Dɩ sobɔr mɩ so nar, paar fɛʋʋkɛ wa-n mɩɩnɩ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ thɩɩraakɛ fɛʋ, wa-n mɩɩrɛ dakha gɩrɛɛkɛ khɛrɩkɛ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ dɩ wa jɩnaa.
40026014	Le kpãkpãadaar bɩɛl yʋɔr yenyɔra, kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Judasɩ, kɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ dɩɩra, jal bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnaa pa a so war ayɩ:
40026015	Anye na tu na ha mɩ, ado mɩ liirna Jeju a ha nɩ? Dɩ wɩ haarɛ wire kpelẽ yʋɔr lɩmɩnɛɛ war.
40026016	Dɩ a fʋna ɔbɔɔlera, a jɩɛ ma da-n ƴaal hʋɛ waa mɔ̃ a na fʋnɩ sɩ aliirna Jeju a ha wɩ.
40026017	Buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraa caca fɛtɩ wi daan, dɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ pɔr Jejura a bulee ayɩ: Kana fɩ-n ƴaal sɩ jala gbɛbɩrɛ Pakɩ dɩkor fɩ kho?
40026018	Dɩ so war: Nɩ jala dɩɩra kũu bɩɛlɩ pa a sʋɔraa ayɛ: Dɩɩrdaar sɔ ayɩwɔɔ aa, ɩnɩ bɔ daan, dɩ afɩ pa ɩna cʋʋ Pakɩ nakha ɩnɩ kpãkpãadara.
40026019	Dɩ kpãkpãadara cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛ Jeju kɔɔ so warnɩ a jal gbɛbɩ Pakɩ dɩkor.
40026020	A dɩɩ dʋɔr, Jeju pɔr na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ, dɩ wɩ too dɩko kho paar.
40026021	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ dɩko khoro, a so warɛ ayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra na liirna mɛr.
40026022	Dɩ wɩ gbobire jɔɔ ka, sa ma fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl dɩ wa-n bule: Mɛr gɩ ya Kɔ̃tɩn?
40026023	Dɩ birse wi: Ʋrɛɛkɛɛ nyɔ̃ n 'lɔɔnɩ kha na mɛrɛ tasa bɩɛl, ɔr gɩɩkɛ na lirena mɩnɩ.
40026024	Mɛr tibili Bikuun wer n jaal mɔ̃ gɩ khere marnɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra, sɩ ga puure tibil ʋrɛraakɛ na lirenanɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun. A wa kɔɔ kɔ̃ tibil ca olelaka', gɩ ka baar.
40026025	Dɩ Judasɩɩkɛ na lirenaanɩ bulee: Dɩ mɛr gɩ ya Dɩɩrdaar? Dɩ Jeju birsee: Gɛrra fɩ so gele.
40026026	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ dɩko khoro Jeju gbaar buru, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a kuure a ha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara sa so war: Nɩ gba a khɔ, gɩrɛra dʋɔn ɩ̃ tomɩ.
40026027	Agɩpɩ dɩ gba thɩ̃ yɔnanɛ, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a fʋɔrnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a ha wɛr sa so war: Nɩ gba fɛʋ a yɔ.
40026028	Gɩdonɩ gɛrra dɔ ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃, Thãgbaa nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ tɔmɩ̃ gɩɩkɛ deerenɩ gɩ faa tɩbɩla bərəəm sopugo.
40026029	Mɩ so narɛ ma bir na yɔ dɩvɛ̃ɛkɛ bã, phaphapha gɩ dana wireekɛ ma birni na yɔ daphaa wo na nɛrɛ ɩ̃ Thɩɩ fãgadaar dɩra.
40026030	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ khɩnɩ nɩɛ pɩ, wɩ ther jal gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra.
40026031	Le Jeju so war ayɩ: Nĩ dɩtɩnɔɔkɛ ɩ̃da na dor nɔɔ dɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ na kɛrna khiru, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Mɛr Thãgba na bɩɩrɛ bana khedaar, dɩ banaasɔɔkɛ gbɛbanɩ kha na bɩ̃bɩlanɛ paar fɛʋ.”
40026032	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɛr Jeju na ɩɩrnɩ na the khirera na pɩ, ma kʋʋl nɛr ƴɩɛ na jal Galile.
40026033	Dɩ Pɩɛr sʋʋraa: Ado afɩda na dor nɔɔ dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na kɛrna khirurakɛ, sɩ me wer ma kɛrna khiru kpɩɩraka'.
40026034	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Sobɔr mɩ so far, fɛrɛ, nĩ dɩtɩnɔɔkɛra yɔl kʋʋ na 'lɛ na khɩɩ pa', sɩ balãther fa bana nayɩ fa jɩ ma'.
40026035	Pɩɛr bir birsee: Adorakɛ wɩ yɩ foo sɩ khe kha, sɩ ma puno na bana nayɩ ma jɩ faa ga. Dɩ ɔmɛna kpãkpãadara fɛʋ so wer.
40026036	Dɩ Jeju kpar ɔɔ kpãkpãadara dɩ wɩ jal da paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jɛcɛmanɛ, dɩ a so warɛ ayɩ: Nɩ tɔɔ kɩɛr ɔbɔɔkɛ ma jalnɩ ma-n bɩɛl Thãgba.
40026037	Dɩ a kɔɔ kpar Pɩɛr na Jebedee bikona yenyɔ, sɩ a mar da-n gbobi dɩ haar kʋɛsʋʋ.
40026038	Dɩ a so warɛ: ɩ̃ ha gbobire khikhi gbobire waa gel. Nɩ tɔɔ kɩɛr a na jʋrɛ na mɛrɛ.
40026039	Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ tɔ jal gbe, a ji thɩɩra a sumo, da-n bɩɛl Thãgba thakɛ ayɩ: ɩ̃ Thɩ, ado hʋɛ na hale, hʋnɔnɛna mɩ thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ, sɩ ga-n do mɔ̃kɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ ga, sɩ mɔ̃kɛ fɛrɛ n pɛrnɩ haar gɩ hana.
40026040	Dɩ agɩpɩ dɩ ɩɩr a bir pɔ kpãkpãadaraa pa a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa-n daar, dɩ so Pɩɛrra: Na kɔɔ puno toorakɛ gbe a jʋʋr hɩɩn na mɛrɛaa koe?
40026041	Na-n jʋrɛ a na bɩɛlna Thãgba, dɩ mɛ̃ na lõ fifiləlela ga. Tuur wer n har haarra gel, sɩ tibili tibil do pa fãga 'lee.
40026042	Dɩ a bire jal balanyɔ wo da-n bɩɛl Thãgba thakɛ ayɩ: Ɩ̃ Thɩ, ado hʋɛ na hale, dɩ thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ na hʋnɔna mɩ sɩɩ do ma yɔ ga, dɔ gɩ ha mɔ̃ fɩ tuni.
40026043	Sɩ a bire pɔ wo a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa-n daar wo, gɩdonɩ dayuur fʋ wɛr a kar.
40026044	Dɩ a faa wɛr sa bir jal da-n bɩɛl Thãgba gɩ do balãther; dɩ mɔna a-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba, thɩmɩɩ nɔ bɩɛlɩlera a bir da-n 'loro.
40026045	Agɩpɩ dɩ bir pɔ kpãkpãadaraa pa a so war: Nɩ daarɛ dɩphã a hɩrɛ. Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã bɔɔ daan dɩ wa fʋ mɛr tibili Bikuun na ha sopugodara.
40026046	Nɩ ɩrɛ sɩ jal, sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ ʋrɛra lirena mɩnɩ n ɩnɛ.
40026047	Dɩ mɔna Jeju hanɩ mɩɩrɔ, Judasɩɩkɛra dɔnɩ bɩɛl kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔra daan, na tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ fɔrɔnɩ bajɩnasɔ, na gbolasɔ, kɛ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na tɩbɩlaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ thɔnɩ.
40026048	Sɩ lĩlir kɔɔ nɩ warɛ gɩrɛ a na cʋʋnɩ aa, ʋrɛɛkɛ ɩna palnɩ, ɔr gɩ, wɩ fʋɔnɛɛ.
40026049	Dɩ dapaara a tɔr dã Jeju sa so: Dɩɩrdaar, gba fʋɔrɛ; sa palʋʋ.
40026050	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Ɩ̃ kuun, gɩrɛ fɩ ɩnɩ fɩ cʋʋ, cʋɛ bɛɛ. Le tɩbɩlaale kpa Jeju a fʋ.
40026051	Dɩ bɩɛl wɩrɛraakɛ hananɩ kha Jeju hal ɔɔ bajɩna, a phe a cɩna gbõdaarɩ thɔ̃daar nũu a kur.
40026052	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Birəna afɩ bajɩna tʋɔr khal kpara, gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na gbaannɩ bajɩna, bajɩnana wa gba na kʋʋrna wɩ.
40026053	Fa jɩ dɩɩ do mɩ hananɛ hʋɛ na bɩɛl ɩ̃ Thɩra da thɔna mar dapaara ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ, dɩ wa ka gbɩlanɩ kpalãther yʋɔr yenyɔra gaa?
40026054	Sɩ a mɩ cʋʋ mɛ̃, mɔ̃ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ ayɩ: Gɩ dana thakɛra, mɔ̃ ga fʋ sɩ na dã na ha oti?
40026055	Ga bɔɔlera Jeju so tibil jɔraale: Nɩ ɩnanɛ bajɩnasɔ na gbolasɔ, nɩ fʋ mɩ mɔ̃ wɩ-n fʋnɩ yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaar koe. Wire fɛʋ mɩ-n kɔɔ toore Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna dɩ ma-n dɩɩr thɩ̃ɛ, sɩ na kɔɔ fʋ ma'.
40026056	Sɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ thakɛ fɛʋ daan, dɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ kherenɩ na dã na ha oti. Le ɔɔ kpãkpãadarasɔ fɛʋ fagʋʋ sa fuule.
40026057	Dɩ wɩrɛ fʋɔnnɩ Jeju, wɩ kpaarɛ jalna Kaɩfɩ gbõdaarɩ pa, ka jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ kpanɩ kha a jɛ.
40026058	Sɩ Pɩɛr n kɔɔ kpar Jejura nɔ bɩɛl nɔ bɩɛl, a ba dana gbõdaarɩ gbaya, a lõ a too le na gardɛsɔ a hɩɩn mɔ̃ ga pɩnɩ.
40026059	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na so gʋʋrdara fɛʋ kɔɔ kpɛr sɔ dɩ wa-n pɛ Jejura, wɩ yɩrɔ hʋɛ wɩ kʋʋ.
40026060	Sɩ wa kɔɔ yɩ ga, sɩrakɛ tibil jɔ kɔɔ pɔr a kuur sɔ̃sɔ dɩ wa-n pɛ Jejura. Pɩpɩɩ paar yenyɔ pɔr a so ayɩ:
40026061	Kuunikɛ sor ayɩ, ɩna punone na wɩɛr Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, sɩ ɩnɩ-n bir ɩnɩ-n mɩ wo wire balãther.
40026062	Dɩ gbõdaar pal ɩɩr a bule Jeju: Fa hana nʋɔ na birsena gaa? Anyee so ha gɩrɛ tɩbɩlaakɛra n pɛ farnɩ thakɛ?
40026063	Sɩ Jeju pɩr pɔbɩ, dɩ gbõdaar bir sʋʋraa: Na Thãgba yidaarɩ i, sɔ sar ado fɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti Thãgbaa Bikuun.
40026064	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Gɛrra ha gele fɩ sonɩ, sɩ wo mɩ so narɛ, a fʋna nɛnɛ̃kɛ na yɩrɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun dɩphã dɩ ma too Thãgbaa nyɔ̃bɔra, dɩ ma ther dakha thãgbara ƴũ ma-n ɩ̃ ndɔlɔ̃panana.
40026065	Le gbõdaar ɓəər ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ sa so: A kʋɛrɛ Thãgbaa i. Anye hale dɩ sa bir na ƴaal so jɩdara 'lo? Mee nɩ nɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ a kʋɛnɩ Thãgbaa i, mɔ̃ nɩ-n kpɩɛr?
40026066	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Khir a teena.
40026067	Sɩ agɩpɩ wɩ mar a cɩɩr nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ dɩ wa-n pɩɛraa ƴɩɛra, sɩ dɩ wa-n thʋʋrʋʋ na nyɔ̃ po, sɩ ɩkhasɔ na-n ɓaalɛɛ sɩ dɩ wa-n so:
40026068	Kirisiti, jɛ ntɛsɔ n bɛ fɩnɩ sa sɔ sar.
40026069	Sɩ Pɩɛr kɔɔ hale a too le phiilo gbayara. Dɩ thɔ̃daar khɛ bɩɛl tɔr pʋɔraa a sʋʋraa: Fɛrɛ dakha, mee fɩ kɔɔ har kha na Galile Jejuukɛra.
40026070	Sɩ a bananɛ awɩ ƴɛra fɛʋ ayɩ: Ma jɩ gɩrɛ fɩ-n ƴaalnɩ fɩ so tɔra'.
40026071	Sɩ agɩpɩ a tɔr thɔɔ lõfonʋɔ, dɩ khɛ kpɩɩ yɩɩ a so wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩle ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ dakha, a-n kɔɔ har kha na Najarɛtɩ Jejura.
40026072	Sɩ a bire bana wo da-n ʋlfɛna ɓoɓo ayɩ: Ma jɩ kuunile kpɩɩraka'.
40026073	Bɔɔ gbe dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ hanɩle tɔr pɔ Pɩɛrra wo a bir sʋʋraa: Sobɔr gɩ gel, fɛrɛ dakha fɛr dɔ waa tibil ca bɩɛl, gɩdonɩ afɩ nɔ mɩɩ wɩ-n jɩna fɩ.
40026074	Le a ma dɩphã da-n wɩɩr thɩ̃ɛsɔ da-n ʋlfɛna ayɩ: Ma jɩ kuunile kpɩɩraka'. Dɩ dapaara yɔl kʋʋ khɩɩ,
40026075	dɩ Pɩɛr jɩnanɛ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ Jeju kɔɔ sʋʋraanɩ: Yɔl kʋʋ na 'lɛ na khɩɩ pa', sɩ fa bananɛ balãther nayɩ fa jɩ ma'. Dɩ le a the khuirə da-n bɩ sɔsɔsɔ.
40027001	A dɩɩ wɩl duuro phiphi, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ fɛʋ na tɩbɩlaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kpar kha a gʋʋr sɩ wɩ kʋ Jeju.
40027002	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ liini pɩ, wɩ kpaarɛ jalna a ha Pɩlatɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ gobanɛr.
40027003	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Judasɩɩkɛ lirenaanɩ yɩnɩ mɔ̃ wɩ pɩɛraanɩ so kʋnanɛ, ɔɔ ha fɛʋ kʋɛrɛ, dɩ gba wire kpelẽ yʋɔr thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ warɩle, a jalna bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnaa pa na tɩbɩlaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ pa a so ayɩ:
40027004	Sopugo mɩ cʋʋ, mɔ̃ mɩ liirnanɩ tibilikɛra na hananɩ dɩ paara' a pɛ khirrə. Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Ga ba sa', fɛr gɩ ba.
40027005	Dɩ Judasɩ gba warɩle a jalna dʋna Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, sa gba jal a ju pɔ̃ɔ.
40027006	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna gbaar warɩle sa so: Ga tee kha dɩ sa gba warɩkɛra na pɛ Thãgba mũsumona ga, gɩdonɩ tibil tɔmɩ̃ the nʋɔ gɩ;
40027007	ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ gʋʋrnɩ khasɔ pɩ, wɩ gbaar warra a thena bʋla mɩdaarra lɩɛ gɩ do kpakpal khi dʋ paar.
40027008	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ wa-n we lɩɛɛle tɔmɩ̃ lɩɛ a dana nĩkɛ.
40027009	Le gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa bobon Jeremɩ kɔɔ sonɩ dã ayɩ: “Wɩ gbaar wire kpelẽ yʋɔr thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ war, kɛ dɔnɩ lɩmɩ nʋɔɔkɛ ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsana gʋʋrnɩ kha dɩ wa thenaa;
40027010	Wɩ kɔɔ gba gɛr a thena bʋla mɩdaarra lɩɛ, mɔ̃kɛra Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ so marnɩ.”
40027011	Dɩ Jeju jɩɩlɛ gobanɛrɩ ƴɛra, dɩ gobanɛr bulee thakɛ ayɩwɔɔ: Fɛr dʋɔn Juifi fãgadaarɩ? Dɩ Jeju birsee: Gɛrra ha gele fɩ sonɩ.
40027012	Sɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔ sookɛ wɩ-n pɩɛraanɩ, aa dee war nʋɔa'.
40027013	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ sʋʋraa: Fa nɩɛ sɔsɔɔkɛra fɛʋ wɩ-n pɛ farnaa?
40027014	Sɩ Jeju na deeraarakɛ nʋɔ thɩ̃ bɩɛlla ga, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ kpaarɛ gobanɛr nʋɔ ka.
40027015	Sɩ fɛtɩra fɛʋ gobanɛr mɩlna gɛr dɩ faa khaɩdaar dɔɔkɛ tibil jɔ n ƴaalnɩ.
40027016	Sɩ kũu ca ʋkha gɩ a kɔɔ hale khaɩra, kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Barabasɩ.
40027017	Mɔ̃ tibil jɔ kpanɩ kha a jɛ, Pɩlatɩ bule wer ayɩ: Ʋmɔ̃ nɩ-n ƴaal gɩrɛra ɩ̃ faa, Barabasɩ gɩ yaa, Jejuukɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Kirisiti gɩ?
40027018	Gɩdonɩ a jɩrɛ dɩ gbugi dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ wɩ fʋ Jeju a haa.
40027019	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a toonɩ ɔɔ kɩɩl too pa, ɔɔ khɛr thʋɔn sʋʋraa: Fa-n lõ tɩɩ sarʋʋlee sora ga, gɩdonɩ ɔɔda dor nɔɔ nĩkɛ dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ gaarɛ dəəlela ka.
40027020	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ n yɩrnanɛ tibil jɔɔle wɩ bɩɛlnɛɛ a faa Barabasɩ sa kɔ Jeju.
40027021	Dɩ gobanɛr bire ɩɩrna gɩ wo a bule wi: Wɛr yenyɔraakɛ, ʋmɔ̃ nɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ faa ha nɩ? Dɩ wɩ birsee, Barabasɩ ɩnɩ-n ƴaal.
40027022	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ bir bule wi: Sɩ anye ma cʋʋna Jejuukɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Kirisiti? Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ so ayɩ: Gbanɛɛ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
40027023	Dɩ gobanɛr bir bule wi: Anyee puu ca a cʋʋ? Dɩ wɩ bir jɩɩ hulẽ wo dɩɩ khɩɩr ka a jɔ mɛ̃ ayɩ: Gbanɛɛ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
40027024	Mɔ̃ Pɩlatɩ yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do aa-n ma gara' sɩ dɩ khʋ̃ɛ bo dɩ ga-n jɔr ka, a gbaar nyʋɔn a hul nyɛ̃ɛ tibil jɔɔlee ƴɛra fɛʋ, sa so ayɩ: Aɩ, tɩɩ sarʋʋ tɔmɩ̃ɩkɛ na-n ma maa koe, nɛr gɩ ba.
40027025	Dɩ tɩbɩlaale fɛʋ so: Ɔɔ, ɔɔ khi thɩmɩɩra n 'le sɩ le na asɩ bɩsãsɔ.
40027026	Le Pɩlatɩ faa Barabasɩ a ha wɩ, sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a ciilni Jeju na khasa pɩ, a fagʋʋrɛ wɩ gbaanɛɛ a kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
40027027	Dɩ gobanɛr sɔrasɩsɔ kpar Jeju a lona gobanɛrɩ cɔ, dɩ sɔrasɛsɔ fɛʋ jɛ a kpalalaa.
40027028	Dɩ wɩ thʋbʋʋrɛ ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ sa gba darã sɩɛ kpɩ̃kpɩ̃kpɩ̃ a tʋʋ,
40027029	sa gba uu a kɛr dɩɩ ho fãgadaar kpɩɛr dɩ wɩ subuu yʋɔ, sa gba ɓalʋʋ a haa dɩ fʋrɔ na nyɔ̃bɔɔ. Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ wɩ gulẽga ɔɔ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn sɩ wa-n maanʋʋ ayɩ: Gba fʋɔrɛ Juifi fãgadaar.
40027030	Sɩ dɩ wɩ cɩɩrna nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ a na pɩɛraa sa tee ɓalʋʋlera dɩ wa-n bɩɩrnaa yʋʋ.
40027031	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ maanʋʋnɩ pɩ, wɩ thʋbʋʋrɛ daraana, sa bir gba ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ a tʋʋ, sa kpaa dɩphã wa-n jalna wɩ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
40027032	Mɔ̃ wɩ-n thenɩ, wɩ caananɛ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ thɛnɩ Sɩrɛn, ɔɔ i n dʋɔn Sɩmɔ̃. Dɩ wɩ cʋgʋʋrɛ na fãga dɩ gba Jejuu kʋkʋ thɩr a heen.
40027033	Dɩ mɔ̃ wɩ danɩ paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Gɔlgɔta, kɩrʋ dʋɔn Yʋ khubu,
40027034	wɩ gbaar dɩvɛ̃ a nyanyaana tomɩ dibi thɩɩ a haa a yɔ. Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a 'lɛnɩ hɩɩn, a bor yʋɔr.
40027035	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ gbaanɩ a kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra pɩ, wɩ gbaar ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ a tɩnɛ na lɩ lɩr.
40027036	Agɩpɩ wɩ toore le dɩ wa-n bɛrʋʋ.
40027037	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ kherere sɛbɛ a ɓã le kʋkʋ thɩrʋra ƴũ ɔɔ yʋɔ, gɩ nɩna ɔɔ so heen kɩr, gɩ sor aa: Ʋrɛɛkɛra dʋɔn Juifi fãgadaar.
40027038	Yu hɔ̃hɔla yenyɔ kɔɔ hale dɩ wɩ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra nakha Jejura, bɩɛl ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra, bɩɛl ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɩlana.
40027039	Wɩrɛ n thɛnɩ le sɩ dɩ wa-n ka, wɩ-n nɩɩrʋʋrɛ, dɩ wa-n didiəna yʋʋ, sɩ dɩ wa-n so aa:
40027040	Fɛrkɛra kɔɔ yɛnɩ, fa wɩɛrɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ sɩ fɩ bir fɩ mɩ wire balãther, taa afɩbara bɛɛ. Ado Thãgbaa Bikuun fɩ do, gbuno kʋkʋ thɩrʋrara.
40027041	Mɛ̃ dakha bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ n ɓoɓororaa, dɩ wa-n sona ayɩ:
40027042	A kɔɔ taarɛ wɩ̃ tibilsɔ, sɩ aa puno na taa dɩbara ga. Dɔ ɔrkɛ dɔnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa fãgadaar n gbũ nɛnɛ̃ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra sɩ pɩɛ haar.
40027043	Mee Thãgba ayɩ, ɩnɩ faarɔrɛ ɩnɩbara, dɩ Thãgbara ado a naarɛ a tagaa nɛnɛ̃ bɛɛ. Gɩdonɩ a-n sor dɩ yɩ: Ɩnɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun.
40027044	Dɩ yu hɔ̃hɔlaakɛ wɩ kpanaanɩ kha n nɩɩrʋʋrɛ dakha wer.
40027045	A fʋna ʋlkhɔɔ a dana dʋɔrɔ, dɩɩ koo kɔɔ birəre tĩtĩtĩ.
40027046	Dɩ dʋɔr khʋra Jeju hulene nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ: Elɩ, Elɩ lama sabakɩtanɩ, kɩrʋ dʋɔn: Ɩ̃ Thãgba, ɩ̃ Thãgba, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fɩ bo mɩ faa?
40027047	Dɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ hanɩle a nɩɛ, wɩ sor aa: Elɩ a-n we.
40027048	Dɩ dapaara tibil bɩɛl wɛrra ca, a gba thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hɔnɩ tabɩhʋɛ, a mʋʋ ta ƴʋɔna, a gar ɓalʋʋ a 'laaraa a yɔ.
40027049	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ so ayɩ: Nɩ dɔ sɩ hɩɩn, ado Elɩra na ɩnɛ na tagʋʋ.
40027050	Sɩ Jeju bire hulẽ wo dɩɩ khɩɩr ka, sa gba ɔɔ thu a ha Thãgba.
40027051	Dɩ hɩnɛ, kẽkẽ nɩɩkɛ varanɩ le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna ɓəəre a tɩnɛ yenyɔ a fʋ ƴũ a ba dana thɩɩ; dɩ dakha thɩɩ jɩɩn kɔɔ hale, dɩ boka kɔ̃tɩnasɔ lɩɛr;
40027052	dɩ kaasɔ dakha khɛr, dɩ tɩɩ phuusɔ jɔɔkɛ kɔɔ khireni ɩɩr a thɩɩr khirera.
40027053	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ a the khirera pɩ, wɩ thɩɩrɛ kaʋ, a lõ dɩ phuurə a nɩna awɩbara tibil jɔjʋɔ.
40027054	Dɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ na wɩrɛ kɔɔ hanaanɩ kha, kɛ jɩlɛnɩ le dɩ wa-n bɛr Jejura, mɔ̃ wɩ yɩnɩ mɔ̃ thɩɩ jenɩ na gɩrɛ dananɩ, maar fʋlɛ wɛr ka dɩ wɩ so: Sobɔr gɩ, kuunikɛra Thãgbaa Bikuun a do ger.
40027055	Dɩ khɛra jɔɔ kɔɔ hale dakha a jɩɩl ƴɔɔ dɩ wa-n hɩɩn. Wɛr dɔ khɛraakɛ n kɔɔ kpaannɩ Jejura dɩ wa-n buluu, a fʋna Galile.
40027056	Khɛrasɔraale, Magɩdala Marɩ kɔɔ hale na Marɩ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ Jakɩ na Jojɛfɩɩ nɩ, na Jebedee bikuunsɔɔ nɩ.
40027057	A dɩɩ dʋɔr lẽle kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jojɛfɩ, kɛ thɛnɩ Arɩmate pɔr. Jejuu kpãkpãadaar a do dakha.
40027058	Dɩ a kɔɔ jaal Pɩlatɩɩ pa a bɩɛlaa Jejuu for, dɩ Pɩlatɩ 'laa hʋɛ wɩ hanaa.
40027059	Dɩ Jojɛfɩ gbaar Jejuu for a parna kẽkẽ ɓɔ̃ bulo phaa,
40027060	a jalna dʋ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ ka phaaraakɛ wɩ kɔɔ thelnɩ gɔ̃gʋɔna. Agɩpɩ dɩ kpuro boka kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ tə̃ə a khaanna ka nʋɔ sa jal kɔ̃.
40027061	Marɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Magɩdala, na Marɩ kpɩɩ hale a too ka nʋɔra.
40027062	A dɩɩ wɩl a thɩɛna gaa gbɛbɩ cɔ wire, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kpar kha a jɛ Pɩlatɩɩ pa,
40027063	a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩ jɩnanɛ fɩfɩɩldaarɩkɛra mɔ̃ a kɔɔ sonɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ yire ayɩ, a wire yẽther ka, ɩna ɩɩrɛ na the khirera.
40027064	Gɛr gɩ, sɔ wa-n bɛr kaa gɩ dana wire yẽther wireelera, a mɛ̃ gaa ɔɔ kpãkpãadara na jaal na yu Jejuu forra na ti, sɩ na so tɩbɩlala nayɩ: A ɩɩrɛ a the khirera. Dɩ pɩpɩɩ fɩɩlɛɛkɛ na puurore na jɔ cacadaa.
40027065	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ so war: Mee mɩ ha nɛr bɛbɛra, nɩ jala na bɛra mɔna nɩ yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ ha.
40027066	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ jal a pɛr dɩ wa-n bɛr kaa, sɩ jɩɩn wɩ pɛr ka nʋɔra, sɩ dɩ bɛbɛra jɩɩl dɩ wa-n bɛr.
40028001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ hɩɩr wire pɩnɩ, ga cʋɔ wi duuro phiphiphi, kɛ dɔnɩ wire makonyɔɔ caca wi, Marɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Magɩdala, na Marɩ kpɩɩlera jaal wɩ hɩɩn kaa.
40028002	Dɩ hɩnɛ, thɩ jẽ kɔ̃ɩĩɩ kɔɔ hale, gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl kɔɔ ther Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ, a kpuro bokaar faa sa tooro.
40028003	Ɔɔ thɛthɛ n carbararɛ a ho mɔ̃ thãgba n lenɩ dɔɔ, dɩ ɔɔ kẽkẽ bulole phɩphɩphɩl a ho mɩlɛ.
40028004	Dɩ maar kɔɔ fʋlɛlɛ gardɛsɔɔle dɩɩ ka, dɩ wɩ ma dɩ wa-n jẽ a thʋ̃ debi a ho khe.
40028005	Sɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurə sor khɛraraale ayɩ: Ado ne wer gɩ, na-n do maar n fʋ na', gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩrɛ Jejuukɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpanɩ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra nɩ-n ƴaal;
40028006	aa haka', a ɩɩrɛ a the khirera mɔna a kɔɔ sonɩ. Nɩ ɩna hɩnɛ kãkɛ wɩ kɔɔ pɩɛnɩ,
40028007	sa jala kɔrɔ a sɔ ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɛ, a ɩɩrɛ a the khirera, dɩ a kʋʋl nɛr ƴɩɛ gɩrɛ da-n jal Galile, le na yɩɩ. Nɩ hɩnɛ, gɛr mɩ jɩ a so nar.
40028008	Dɩ dapaara wɩ faarɛ kaa sa gba wa-n jal na jẽu na da kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, sɩ kpãkpãadara wɩ ca jal a mɩɩ thɩ̃ɛɛlera.
40028009	Dɩ hɩnɛ, Jeju pɔr a caan wɩ a so: Mɩ fʋɔr nɛr. Dɩ khɛraale tɔr wɔrɔ̃ɔ a palʋʋ nɛɛ, dɩ wa-n fʋɔrʋʋ.
40028010	Dɩ Jeju so warɛ ayɩ: Na-n do maar n fʋ na', sɩ nɩ jala sɔ ɩ̃ omisɔra wa-n jala Galile, le wa yɩ mɩ.
40028011	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ khɛraale kɔɔ hanɩ hʋɛra wa-n jal, wɩ̃ kũusɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ bɛbɛraale kɔɔ jaal dɩɩra a mɩɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋle kɔɔ dananɩ.
40028012	Dɩ wɛr, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kpanɩ kha na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ a gʋʋr pɩ, wɩ gbaar war jɔɔ a ha sɔrasɛɛle sa so war ayɩ:
40028013	Nɩ sɔ ayɛwɔɔ: Ɔɔ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ pʋɔn dɩtɩnɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ-n daarnɩ, a yuu ti.
40028014	Dɩ ado gobanɛr nɩɛ, sa dor bʋɔ na cʋgʋʋ da tu gɩ do nɔɔ na 'lɛ sora'.
40028015	Dɩ sɔrasɛsɔ gbaar warɩle, sa cʋʋ mɔna wɩ kɔɔ so warnɩ wɩ cʋɛ. Dɩ thɩmɩɩ ca gelera kpaarɛ Juifisɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn a dana nĩkɛ.
40028016	Dɩ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr bɩɛl jaal Galile, gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ Jeju kɔɔ yɩnɩ wɩ caanɛ nɩ.
40028017	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ, wɩ gburõkure dɩ wa-n fʋɔrʋʋ. Sɩ ɩkhasɔ wɛrra bor sɩ wa-n baalɔ.
40028018	Dɩ Jeju tɔr pɔ war sa so war thakɛ ayɩwɔɔ: Fãga fɛʋ, mɛr Thãgba ha, thãgbara ƴũ a gbana thɩɩra.
40028019	Gɛr gɩ nɩ jala caarra fɛʋ a na cʋɛ tɩbɩla wɩ do kpãkpãadara. Nɩ gba Thɩrɛ, na Bikuun, na Thu Phuu i a na kpɛana wɩ nyʋɔnɔ;
40028020	dɩ na-n dɩrɛ wɩ wa-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ kɔɔ so narnɩ. Sɩ hɩnɛ, mɛrɛ ma-n har kha na nɛrɛ wire wo wire fɛʋ, gɩ dana thɩɩkɛ pɩ wi.
41001001	Kɩɛr gɩ fʋ dɩ a-n mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Thãgbaa Bikuun Jeju Kirisitiida,
41001002	mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩ kɔɔ kherenɩ ɔɔ sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Hɩnɛ, mɛr Thãgba thɔna ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃, dɩ na kʋʋl fɩ ƴɩɛ, a gbɛbɩ afɩ hʋ.
41001003	Tibil wire gɩ dɩ ga-n hulẽ bəənnə ayɩ: Na-n gbɛbɩrɛ hʋɛ Kɔ̃tɩnna, na-n wɛbɩrɛ ɔɔ hʋ bisɔ gɩ pɔlɔ.”
41001004	Mɛ̃ Jã ɩɩr bəənnə da-n kpɛɛ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ da-n sona war ayɩ: Nɩ deba haar sa 'lɛ yɔ kpɛɛrɛ sɩ Thãgba n faa nɩ sopugosɔ.
41001005	Dɩ tɩbɩla n kɔɔ ther Jude dɩɩra fɛʋ na Jerujalɛm dɩ wa-n pʋɔraa, dɩ wɩ cã awɩ sopugosɔ sɩ dɩ Jã na-n kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔ Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩrra.
41001006	Nyɔɔmɛɛ sũu wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋna Jãa kẽkẽekɛ a-n tonɩ dɩ linə lophɛrɛ pelela, sɩ toosõo na thʋʋr n kɔɔ dɔ ɔɔ dɩko.
41001007	Sɩ da-n mɩɩ tɩbɩla ayɩ: Bɩɛl hale na kpa mar, a hana fãga a jɔ mɩ, dɩ ma hɩɩrʋʋrakɛ a na thʋbʋʋ nɛfaa pɛ̃a'.
41001008	Me wer nyʋɔnɔ mɩ kpɛɛ nɩ, sɩ ɔr, Thu Phuurə a na kpɛɛ nɩ.
41001009	Ɔbɔɔlera Jeju kɔɔ the Najarɛtɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Galile dɩɩ a pɔ, dɩ Jã kɔɔ kpɛgʋʋ nyʋɔnɔ Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩrra.
41001010	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ a-n thenɩ nyʋɔnɔ, a yɩrɛ thãgbara ƴũ dɩɩ phubi bə̃, dɩ Thu Phuu gbũ a ho puusɩ̃ɛ a lʋʋnaa.
41001011	Dɩ nʋɔ the thãgbara ƴũ a so: Fɛr dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, fɩ lõ mer haar kpɛ.
41001012	Dɩ dapaara Thu Phuu cʋʋ Jeju dɩ jal bəənnə;
41001013	a too le wire kpalanyɔ dɩ Satã na-n fifiləə, hɔ̃ nʋma a kɔɔ hana kha le, dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ n pɔ dɩ wa-n haa gɩrɛ n danaanɩ.
41001014	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ fʋnɩ Jã a to khaɩra pɩ, gɛr Jeju jaal Galile da-n mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara da-n so ayɩ:
41001015	Wire daan dɩ Thãgba na-n gba fãga. Nɩ deba haar sa pɩɛr tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haar.
41001016	Mɔ̃kɛ Jejura n jalnɩ na Galile mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔ, a yɩrɛ Sɩmɔ̃ na Ãdire, Sɩmɔ̃ɔ õkuunna dɩ wɩ ha dɩ wa-n dʋna thʋ̃ pherdaakɛ n hɔnɩ jɔ̃ mɩɩr nɔɔra, gɩdonɩ thʋ̃ pherdara ha wɩ.
41001017	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju so war: Na-n kpa mar ɩ̃ cʋʋ nɩ na-n ƴaal tɩbɩla thʋ̃ khaa.
41001018	Dɩ dapaara wɩ faarɛ awɩ thʋ̃ pherdasɔ sɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
41001019	Dɩ bir gba na jal gbe, a yɩ Jakɩ na ɔɔ õkuun Jã, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ Jebedee bikona, dɩ wɩ ha gboroona dɩ wa n gbɛbɩ awɩ thʋ̃ pherdasɔ.
41001020	Dɩ dapaara a we wer, dɩ wɩ faa awɩ thɩ Jebede gboroona na thɔ̃dara sɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
41001021	Dɩ wɩ jaal dã Kapɛrnayʋm dɩɩra, dɩ hɩɩr wire Jeju lõ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra a ma da-n dɩɩr wɩ.
41001022	Dɩ nʋɔ kpaa tɩbɩla ɔɔ dɩɩrra gɩdonɩ a-n dɩɩr wɛr mɔ̃ a hananɩ hʋɛ, ga ho mɔ̃ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ n dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla ga.
41001023	Dɩ le wɩ yɩ kũu bɩɛl Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, kɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl hananɩ, dɩ a hulene ayɩ:
41001024	Ee, anye sɩ ha kha na fɛr Najarɛtɩ Jeju? Fɩ ɩnɛ fɩ kʋɛ sɩ ya? Mɩ jɩrɛ ntɛ fɩ donɩ: Thãgbaa Tɩɩ phu fɩ do.
41001025	Sɩ Jeju manaanɛ ayɩ: Pɩra, sa thɛ kuunnaale.
41001026	Mɔ̃kɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔlɩle cʋʋnɩ kuunile dɩ ji da-n laan, a hulene sa the dɩphã.
41001027	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩ wa-n bule khasɔ bɩɛlbɩɛl aa: Anye gɩ ya fɛ? Dɩɩr kpɩɩ gɩ; a-n mar kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔlasɔrarakɛ dɩ puno wi, dɩ wa-n nɩɩ nũu.
41001028	Dɩ ɔɔ i kpaar dapaara Galile dɩɩra fɛʋ.
41001029	Ɔbɔɔle wɩ kɔɔ thenɩ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, wɩ jaal dapaara na Jakɩ na Jã, a lõ Sɩmɔ̃ na Ãdiree cɔ.
41001030	Dɩ Sɩmɔ̃ɔ khɛrɩ nɩ gɩ, a ji tomɩ kporre, dɩ dapaara wɩ sor Jejura.
41001031	Dɩ Jeju pɔ fʋʋ nyɔ̃ɔ, a khəi dɩ ɩɩr, dɩ dapaara tomɩ kporre ɩɩraa dɩ cɛ wɩ nyʋɔn.
41001032	Dʋɔrɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ wire lonɩ pɩ, tɩbɩla kɔɔ gbaar khodara fɛʋ na kpãkpũdara dɩ wa-n pɔna Jejura,
41001033	dɩ dɩdara fɛʋ kɔɔ gbɛbɩrɛ kha dɩ wa-n der cɔ lõfonʋɔra.
41001034	Dɩ a kpɛɛrɛ khodara jɔɔkɛ kho caar dɩɩdɩɩ fʋnɩ dɩ wa-n gaar, sa weena dakha kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ jɔɔ a faa, sɩ aa-n tu kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ n mɩa nʋɔa', gɩdonɩ wɩ jɩɩrɛ.
41001035	Ɔbɔɔkɛ yɔl ko khɩɩ bɔɔ na kɔɔ danɩ pa', gɛr Jeju mãa ɩrɛrɔ a the jal dɩ khuirə, dɩ le a too dɩbara da n bɩɛl Thãgba.
41001036	Dɩ Sɩmɔ̃ na ɔɔ 'walãkhasɔ the jal dɩ wa-n ƴaalʋʋ;
41001037	ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ wɩ sʋʋraarɛ ayɩ: Tɩbɩla fɛʋ n ƴaal fɛr.
41001038	Sɩ Jeju so war: Nɩ ɩna sɩ jal dɩkhãa pa dɩɩraakɛ maanɩ gbe, ɩ̃ mɩɩ le dakha Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ, gɩdonɩ gɛr mɩ ɩnɔ.
41001039	Dɩ mɛ̃ a jal paar fɛʋ Galile dɩɩra, da-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, da-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ da-n faa.
41001040	Gbuuluu gɩ, a pɔ Jejura, a gulẽgaraa da-n phʋʋrʋʋ ayɩ: Ado fɩ ture fɩ punone cʋʋ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ gbuul pɩ.
41001041	Dɩ bʋɔ fʋ Jeju dɩ 'laa nyɔ̃ɔ a thaaraa sa so: Mɩ ture afɩ gbuul n pɛ.
41001042	Dɩ dapaara gbuule pɩɩraa dɩ kpɛɛ.
41001043	Sɩ Jeju sʋʋraarɛ a kɔna sɩ a jɩɛ kpãkpaanaa na sobɔr ayɩ:
41001044	Jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ fa-n so tibillə ga, sɩ jala nɛna Thãgbaa bonɩ jidaar mɔ̃ fɩ hanɩ, sa 'laanɛ phɔphʋɔl thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sonɩ, gɩ nɩna tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩ fɩ kpɛɛrɛ.
41001045	Sɩ kuunile jaal, a ma a be da-n wɩɛl paar fɛʋ gɩrɛ kɔɔ danaanɩ; gelela dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ Jeju na-n puno dɩ lõ dɩ bɩnɔ bã; sɩ dɩ khuirə a-n too kãkɛ tɩbɩla na-n hana', dɩ tɩbɩla n ther paar fɛʋ dɩ wa-n pʋɔraa.
41002001	A wire gbe kɔɔ ka, Jeju bire pɔ Kapɛrnayʋm, dɩ wɩ nɩɛrɛ a hale cʋɔrɔ.
41002002	Dɩ tibil jɔ kɔɔ gbɛbɩ kha der le dɩ a do too paar na yɩrɛ bã, dɩ phiilo gɩrakɛ lõfonɔa'. Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ a-n mɩɩ wɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ,
41002003	tɩbɩla pɔr na gbãgbaʋʋkɛ tɩbɩla yenã heennɩ.
41002004	Sɩ ga do wa punone na dana Jejuu thɛtha', gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla jɔrɛ ka, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ hɩɩnɔ ka Jeju hanɩ sa cu kaar le nãsʋrɔ, sa gba gbãgbarʋra na ɔɔ jɔ̃ a tona kaarra.
41002005	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju yɩnɩ awɩ ha pɛ, a sor gbãgbarʋra ayɩ: Ɩ̃ kuun, afɩ sopugosɔ hɛl farɛ.
41002006	Sɩ wɩ̃ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔɔkɛ hanɩle n sor na awɩ bɩ̃ aa:
41002007	Anyee tibil ca ha ʋrɛ a mɩɩ da-n kʋɛna Thãgbaa i thakɛ? Amɛ n punone dɩ faa sopugo saagado Thãgba gɩ dɩbara ga?
41002008	Dɩ dapaara Jeju jɩ na ɔɔ ha mɔ̃ wɩ-n kpɩɛrnɩ awɩ bɩnɔ a so war: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nɩ hana kpɩɛr caar thale anɩ bɩnɔ?
41002009	Gɩmɔ̃ yɔɔnɛ sorra gbãgbarʋra: Sopugo hɛl farɛ gɩ yaa, agɩbo: Ɩrɛ, gba afɩ jɔ̃ na jala gɩ?
41002010	Sɩ mɩ ƴaalɛ nɩ jɛ dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun hananɛ hʋɛ thɩɩra dɩ ɩ̃ faana sopugo, sa bir so gbãgbarʋra:
41002011	Mɩ so farɛ, ɩrɛ gba afɩ jɔ̃ na kɔna.
41002012	Dɩ dapaara dɩ ɩɩr gba ɔɔ jɔ̃, dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ yɩɩ dɩ sa da-n the, dɩ nʋɔ kpaa wɩ dɩ wa-n khɩɩ Thãgba dɩ wa-n sona ayɩ: Sɩ kɔɔ thenɩ dɩɩra, sa kɔɔ yɩ thɩ̃ɛ thakɛ kpɩɩa'.
41002013	Dɩ Jeju bire kɛr bir mɩɩr nɔɔra, dɩ tibil jɔ na-n pʋɔraa da-n dɩɩr wɩ.
41002014	Sɩ a-n kar a yɩ Levɩ, Alfee bikuun dɩ too war gba paar da-n tee war, dɩ sʋʋraa: Na kpa mar; dɩ ɩɩr da-n kpaaraa.
41002015	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju toonɩ dɩko kho paar Levɩɩ cɔ, war gbadara na sopugodara jɔɔ toonaanɛ na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara dakha, gɩdonɩ wa tibil casɔɔle n kpaaraanɩ wɩ jɔrɛ.
41002016	Dɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ a bir dona jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kɔɔ yɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ Jeju n khonɩ dɩkor na sopugodara na war gbadara, wɩ sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Mɔ̃gɩdo da-n kho dɩkor na war gbadara na sopugodara?
41002017	Dɩ Jeju nɩɛ mɔ̃ wɩ-n sonɩ a so war: Ga do tɩɩ khena n kɔɔ ƴaalɛ dɔtɔrɔa', sɩ wɩrɛ gɩ-n khonɩ gɩ. Ga do tɩɩ sara mɩ ɩ̃ ɩ̃ ƴaala', sɩ sopugodara wɛ.
41002018	Wi bɩɛl mɔ̃kɛ Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ kpãkpãadara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kɔɔ lini nʋɔ, tɩbɩla jaal a bule Jeju: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ kpãkpãadara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraa kpãkpãadara na-n li nʋɔ, sɩ afɩ kpãkpãadara wer na-n li nʋɔa'.
41002019	Dɩ Jeju tu wi: Nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ dɩ wɩrɛ wɩ wenɩ herra na punone na li nʋɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ kha na khɛr he ya? Kpei. Bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ toonanɩ kha khɛr he wa puno na li nʋɔa'.
41002020	Sɩ wire na hale wa hɛl warnɩ khɛr he, dawiile wa li nʋɔ dɩphã.
41002021	Tibil na gba kẽkẽ phaa na coorna kẽkẽ tɩ̃ɩ na bɛba'. A a cʋʋ mɛ̃, daphaa na-n haalɛ datɩ̃ɩ gɩ ɓəər gɩ puuro ga-n pɛr.
41002022	Tibil na gba thʋʋrɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ daphaa na pɛr bʋla tɩɩna ga. A a cʋʋ mɛ̃ thʋʋr na wɩɛlɛ bʋla tɩ̃ɩle, gɩ do thʋʋr na bʋlaa kʋɛrɛ fɛʋ, sɩ dɔ fɩ pɛ thʋ phaa bʋla phaara oti.
41002023	Hɩɩr wi bɩɛl Jeju n kɔɔ kar a lõ jʋ lɩɛra, dɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n jalnɩ na hʋɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara 'laarɛ a kha jɔ a kho.
41002024	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara sʋʋraa: Fa yɩ mɔ̃ afɩ kpãkpãadara n cʋʋnɩ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ yɩnɩ gɩ-n sãsɩrɛ hɩɩr wirəə?
41002025	Dɩ Jeju tu wi: Na kɔɔ yɩɛ sɛbɛra gɩrɛɛkɛ Davɩdɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ ƴaalnɩ dɩkor gɩdonɩ kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋʋrɛ na wɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ kha gaa?
41002026	Mee a kɔɔ lʋʋn Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ Abɩataar kɔɔ donɩ Thãgbaa gbõdaar, a gba buruukɛ wɩ-n hanɩ Thãgba kɛ n sãsɩnɛnɩ tɩɩ khɩnana a kho, a ɩɩr wo a ha tɩbɩlaakɛ a hananɩ.
41002027	Sɩ Jeju bire so war: Tibil Thãgba cʋʋ hɩɩr wire a ha, aa ti tibil a ha hɩɩr wirə'.
41002028	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun do Kɔ̃tɩn hɩɩr wirerarakɛ.
41003001	Agɩpɩ Jeju bir lõ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra wo; dɩ le a yɩ kuunikɛ nyɔ̃ɔ khini.
41003002	Dɩ wɩrɛ hanɩle jʋʋr Jeju dɩ wa-n hɩɩn ado a na kpɛɛrɛ kuunile hɩɩr wire, gɩdonɩ wɩ-n ƴaalɛ wɩ pɛr Jejura sor.
41003003	Dɩ Jeju so kuunnaale nyɔ̃ɔ khini ayɩ: Ɩrɛ jɩlɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
41003004	Sa bir bule wi: Hɩɩr wire teana bɔ cʋʋrɛ yaa puu cʋʋrɛ, agɩbo fɩ taa tibil yaa, fɩ kʋ tibil? Sɩ wɩ pɩrrɛ pɔbɩ.
41003005	Dɩ haar n heluule gɩdonɩ awɩda khɩɩrɛ, dɩ hɩɩn wɩ na nĩkhii da-n finə sa bir so kuunna: 'Laanɛ afɩ nyɔ̃; dɩ 'laa dɩɩ do gɩ kpɛɛrɛ.
41003006	Dɩjɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara the, a gbɛbɩ kha dapaara na Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ too dɩ wa-n gʋʋr mɔ̃ wa fʋnɩ sɩ wɩ kʋ Jeju.
41003007	Sɩ Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara gbaar jal mɩɩr nɔɔra, dɩ tibil jɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃ kɔɔ kpaaraarɛ. Ɩkhasɔ ther Galile, na Jude,
41003008	na Jerujalɛm, na ldume dɩɩra, na Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩr iiro, na Tɩɩr na Sɩdɔ̃ dɩ khʋra. Tibil jɔɔle pɔr Jejura thale gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ wɩ nɩɛ.
41003009	Gɛr gɩ dɩ Jeju so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara wɩ gbɛbɩrɛ nar too paar gboroona a thɩnɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ tɩbɩla na yɩ nɩ gbʋɔr paara'.
41003010	Gɩdonɩ a-n kpɛɛrɛ khodara jɔɔ, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩrɛ gɩ-n khonɩ n hiirəə ɩna-n thaaraa.
41003011	Dɩ bɔɔ wo bɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔla n yɩɩnɩ, wɩ-n jire thʋnɔ ɔɔ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn dɩ wa-n be hulẽbe dɩɩ khɩɩr ka, dɩ wɩ yɩ: Fɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun.
41003012	Sɩ Jeju n kpãkpãa warɛ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka dɩ wa-n so ntɛ ɩnɩ dona'.
41003013	Agɩpɩ Jeju jʋʋn gɔ̃gʋɔna, sa we tɩbɩlaakɛ a-n ƴaalnɩ dɩ wɩ pʋɔraa.
41003014	Dɩ a phiire yʋɔr yenyɔ wa-n ha kha na ɔr a thɔ̃ wɩ wɩ jal wa-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ;
41003015	a ha wɛr dakha punone dɩ wa weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ.
41003016	Yʋɔr yenyɔɔkɛ ha wɩrɛ a phiirni: Sɩmɔ̃ ɔr a dʋ ire Pɩɛr,
41003017	Jakɩ na ɔɔ õkuun Jã, Jebedee bikona wɛ; wɛr Jeju ha ire Boanɛrjɛsɩ, kɩrʋ dʋɔn wɩrɛ n phaanɛnɩ oro'oro thãgba phɛɛ khaa;
41003018	Ãdire, Filipi, Bartelemɩ, Matiə, Tomasɩ, Jakɩ Alfee bikuun, Tade, Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ dʋɔnnɩ gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ tibil,
41003019	na Judasɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ dɩɩra, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ lirenanɩ Jeju.
41003020	Agɩpɩ Jeju kɛr bir kɔ̃ cʋɔrɔ, dɩ tɩbɩla bir wo a gbɛbɩ kha le, dɩ ga do Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara na ba yɩrɛ ƴɩɛrakɛ na kho dɩkora'.
41003021	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ɔɔ too nɩɛnɩ wɩ kɔɔ pɔr wɩ kpaa, gɩdonɩ a thɩɛna gaa wɩ yɩ: Yʋʋ buure.
41003022	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Jerujalɛm a pɔ so ayɩ: Bɛljɛbulikɛ dʋɔnnɩ Satã lʋʋnaanɛ, wo: Ɔrkɛra dɔnɩ yʋʋ kɔ̃tɛɛbiirə n hanaa fãga dɩ weena kɔ̃tɛɛbii.
41003023	Dɩ Jeju we wɩ a so war sokpaakɛ thakɛ ayɩ: Mɔ̃ Satã na puno na wee dɩbara?
41003024	A fãgadaarɩ dɩ bɩɛl tɩnɛ a na ke kha, fãgadaarɩ dɩ dɔɔle na jɩɩla'.
41003025	A cɔ bɩɛl gɩɩkɛ tɩnɛnɛnɩ a na ke kha, cɔ dɔɔle na jɩɩla'.
41003026	A Satã na kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ na ɔɔbara dɩ tɩnɛ paar har ɔɔ fãga dɩra, ɔɔ puno na jal bã sɩ ga pɩrɛ.
41003027	Tibil na puno na lõ na fãga kũu khɩɩ cɔ na taaraa thɩ̃ɛ, saagado ɔr a kɔɔ li ɓoaa ga, a a punoo ɓo dɩphã gɛr a na taaraa thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ cʋɔrɔ.
41003028	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel: Thãgba na faarɛ tɩbɩlaa sopugosɔ fɛʋ na ɔɔ i kʋɛɛkɛ wɩ-n kʋɛnɩ.
41003029	Sɩ tibilikɛ na kʋɛanɩ Thu Phuu i, Thãgba na faa ga sopugo caale yuuraka', sɩ sor na heenuune khorr.
41003030	Jeju mɩɩrɛ thakɛ gɩdonɩ wɩ yɩ: Kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl lʋʋnaanɛ.
41003031	Le Jejuu nɩ na ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔsɔ dã, a jɩɩl phiilo sa thɔ̃ wɩɩ.
41003032	Sɩ tibil jɔ kɔɔ toore a diirəə dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Pɛ nũu, afɩ nɩ na afɩ õkona har phiilo dɩ wa-n bule fi.
41003033	Dɩ tu wi: Amɛ n dʋɔn ɩ̃ nɩ, na ɩ̃ õkona?
41003034	Sɩ a mar a hɩɩn wɩrɛ tɔɔnɩ a diirəə da-n finə sa so: Wɩrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ nɩ na ɩ̃ õkona;
41003035	gɩdonɩ ɩibilikɛ n cʋɛɩɩɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ, wa tibilile dʋɔn ɩ̃ õkuun, na ɩ̃ õkhɛr, na ɩ̃ nɩ.
41004001	Jeju bire a ma wo da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ mɩɩr nɔɔra, dɩ tibil jɔ gbɛbɩ pʋɔraa a der, gɛr hɩna dɩ jʋʋn a too gboroona mɩɩr nɔ nyʋɔnɔ, sɩ dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ too thɩɩra mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔra.
41004002	Dɩ a dɩɩr wɛr thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ na sokpaa, a so warɛ ɔɔ dɩɩrra ayɩ:
41004003	Nɩ pɛ nũu: Bi jaldaar gɩ, a the da-n jal be.
41004004	Mɔ̃kɛ a-n jalnɩ yɛ̃ bi jire hʋɛra, dɩ 'lominə pɔ uul.
41004005	Yɛ ji wo bokanana ka thɩ nʋʋn na jɔrna', a phu dapaara kɔrɔ gɩdonɩ ga jɩɩ mʋʋ a hulõə';
41004006	sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wire phanɩ dɩ ɩtʋɛ hẽ, gɩ ɔ̃'ɔlɔnɛ a khi, gɩdonɩ nɛɛ na hala'.
41004007	Yɛ ji wo ka u nɛɛ hanɩ, dɩ uu ɩɩr a sɩlã gɩ dɩ ga se bə'.
41004008	Yɛ ji thɩ bʋɔra, a phu, a khɔ̃, a bɩ̃, bi bɩɛl n bɩnɛ dɩ hana be kpelẽ yʋɔr, ɩkha kpalãther, ɩkha tamaa.
41004009	Sɩ Jeju so warɛ ayɩ: Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
41004010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ hanɩ kha na tibil jɔɔle bã, wɩrɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ totoosɔ na kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ wɩ buleele sokpaa kɩrra.
41004011	Dɩ so war: Nɛr Thãgba kɔɔ ha nɩ jɛ thɩ̃ gbulikɛ dʋɔnnɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do, sɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ tɩɩ khina, sokpaa thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ do war,
41004012	dɩ mɛ̃, “Wa-n hɩɩn sɩ wa yɩ ga, wa-n nɩɛ dakha sɩ wa jɩ kɩrʋa', a mɛ̃ gaa, ga hor wa kɛrrɛ na bir Thãgbara a na 'lɛ sopugo faarɛ.”
41004013	Sɩ Jeju bire so war wo: Dɩ a na jɩ sokpaakɛ kɩrʋa', mɔ̃ na fʋ sɩ na jɩ gɩ̃ sokpasɔ fɛʋ kɩrʋ?
41004014	Thãgbaa so bi jaldaar n jal.
41004015	Ɩkhaa tibilsɔ hʋrɛ hʋ nʋɔ ka sor kɔɔ jalnɩ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n nɩɛnɩ, Satã n pɔr dapaara dɩ tiir sorɩkɛ kɔɔ direni awɩ hara.
41004016	Mɛna gɩ ha na wɩrɛ hɔnɩ boka thɩɩ ka be kɔɔ jalnɩ. Wɛr dɔ wɩrɛ n nɩɛnɛnɩ Thãgbaa so dɩ wɩ tu na daʋ dapaara,
41004017	sɩ wa-n sɩrɔ Thãgbaa so dɩɩ yɩ nɛ gɔ paar awɩ hara ga. Bɔɔ gbe wɩ-n pər gar dɩbara, sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩwɛ na kpoore n danɩ, dɩɩ do Thãgbaa soolera dɔ nɔɔ, dɩɩ do dapaara wɩ faarɛ ha pɛrɛ.
41004018	Wɛ n nɩɛrɛ Thãgbaa so, sɩ dɩ wɩ ho ka uu hanɩ sɩ be jallɔ;
41004019	sɩ dɩɩ do dɛr bɔɔraakɛra na lẽle thɩ̃ kpɩɛr fifiləle na gɩ̃ ha pɩɛrsɔ, gele n ɩrɛ dɩɩ sɩlã Thãgbaa soolera dɩ ga-n puno na se bə'.
41004020	Wɩrɛ n nɩɛnɛnɩ Thãgbaa so dɩ wɩ tu, wɛr hʋɔn thɩ bʋɔ, ka be kɔɔ jalnɩ dɩɩ do wɩ-n ser be: Bɩɛl n ser kpelẽ yʋɔr, dɩkha kpalãther, dɩkha tamaa bi bɩɛlla.
41004021	Sɩ Jeju bire bule wi wo: Wɩ-n gbaar lãphã pɛ a suuro bɩlãkpʋʋn kã? Dɩ agɩbo dɩ wɩ to kakala ballɔ kã? Mee bilela wɩ-n dɛ̃ɛ.
41004022	Thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ker sɩ ga do wɩ cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ thaa ga; thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ha gbul sɩɩ do ga yɩraa ga.
41004023	Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
41004024	A bire so war wo: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ gɩrɛraakɛ nɩ nɩɛnɩ bʋrɛ; mɩɛda caakɛ nɩ kɔɔ mɩɛnanɩ thɩ̃ɛ, ɔr wa mɩɛna na ha nɩ sɩ na dɛbɩna nar kɔ̃dɩ̃.
41004025	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ hananɩ thɩ̃ɛ, Thãgba na bire na haa na dɛbɩrɔ; sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ thɩ̃a', Thãgba na tiirəərerakɛ phubi gɩrɛɛkɛ a hananɩ.
41004026	Jeju bire a so wo: Thãgbaa fãgadaar do, gɩ hʋrɛ tibilikɛ n jalanɩ be lɔɔ;
41004027	sɩ a a-n daarɛ, a a-n ɩɩrɛ, dɩtɩnɔ na dɩwɩlʋ yo, sɩ gɩ-n phaan phulole dɩɩ phu, sɩ aa-n jɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋna';
41004028	faa thɩɩ thɛthɛ n cʋʋ dɩɩ phu ɓo, agɩpɩ dɩɩ pemi sa hana be dɩphã.
41004029	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ gɩ bɩnɩ pɩ, dapaara dɩɩ do wɩ-n khar gɩdonɩ bɔɔ daan.
41004030	Jeju bire a so war wo aa: Anye sa gba na mɩɛna mɔ̃ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do hanɩ, anyee sokpa ca sa gba na mɩɛna?
41004031	Gɩ hʋrɛ beekɛ wɩ-n wenɩ seneve wɩ-n diirni, fɩɩʋ a-n ha dɩ jɔ be fɛʋ thɩɩra.
41004032	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ diiruuni pɩ, a-n ɩɩrɛ dɩ wabɩ dɩ jɔ thɩr bii fɛʋ; a-n hananɛ jɛ̃ kɔ̃tɩna dɩ 'lominə n puno dɩ wa-n tɛllɔ.
41004033	Sokpa caar thakɛ jɔɔ a-n kɔɔ mɩɩna tɩbɩla Thãgbaa so mɔ̃ wa punoni na nɩɛ;
41004034	aa-n kɔɔ mɩɩna wɩ saagado sokpa gaaga, sɩ a a ha kha na kpãkpãadara dɩbara gɛr a-n mɩɛ war kɩrʋ.
41004035	Ga wiilera dʋɔsɛʋ Jeju so war: Nɩ dɔ sɩ iir iiro.
41004036	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ faa tɩbɩla sa phɛl gborõokɛ a harɔnɩ a jal, sɩ yɛ̃ gborõ kɔɔ hanaanɛ kha.
41004037	Dɩ thãgba jɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ɩɩr na fãga, dɩ nyʋɔn ubi a lõ gboroona, dɩ wa jɩ dɩɩ do gɩ 'lire dɩ ga-n hi gborõo.
41004038	Sɩ Jeju ha gborõ sɩkaar, a jəə yʋʋ da-n daar; dɩ wɩ jagʋʋrɛ a sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar fa-n therna asɩ kʋɛra sɩ-n kʋɛnaa?
41004039	Dɩ mɛ̃ a jaa a mana jɩɛ aa: Pɩra; a sona mɩɩr nɔ nyʋɔnna aa: Jɩlɛ cɔcɔ; dɩ jɩɛ kur dɩ thɩ̃ɛ na hale dɩɩ tutugo bã.
41004040	Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ so war: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ maar fʋ nɩ thakɛ? Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na pɛr Thãgba haara?
41004041	Maar fʋ wɛr na sobɔr sɩ dɩ wa-n bule kha bɩɛlbɩɛl aa: Anyee tibil ca ha ʋrɛ, dɩ jɩɛrakɛ na mɩɩr nɔ nyʋɔn na-n nɩɩ nũu?
41005001	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan mɩɩr nɔ iiro Jerajedaraa dʋɔ.
41005002	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju thenɩ gboroona, dapaara kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl ther khi dʋ paar da-n caanʋʋ.
41005003	Kuunile khi dʋ paar a-n cɔ dɩ dakha tibil na-n puno dɩ lii 'lo bã, jɔrkɔrakɛ na-n puno dɩɩ liə';
41005004	gɩdonɩ wa-n bʋʋ lirə', sɩ wɩ-n kɔɔ baraanɛ na ther dɩ wɩ linəə dakha jɔrkɔ, sɩ a-n kɔɔ hallɛ jɔrkɔ dɩ phʋ̃ dɩ bɛɛna therɩle dɩ khaar, sɩ tibillakɛ na hale dɩ punooə'.
41005005	Bɔɔ fɛʋ, dɩtɩnɔ na dɩwɩlʋ, khi dʋ paarsɔ na gɔ̃gʋɔna a-n ha da-n hulẽ, sɩ dɩ gba bokana da-n liirena tomɩr.
41005006	Dɩ mɔ̃ a 'laanɩ yɩ Jeju ƴɔɔ, a car a caanʋʋ a gburõkuraa,
41005007	sa hulẽ nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ: Anye fɛrɛ na mɛrɛ ha kha, fɛr Jeju Thãgba Kəkəədaarɩ Bikuun? Mɩ-n phʋʋr fɛr na Thãgbaa i, fa-n hʋɔl mara'.
41005008	A sor thale gɩdonɩ Jeju kɔɔ sʋʋraarɛ: Thɛ kuunnaale, fɛr kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl.
41005009	Dɩ Jeju bulee: Mɔ̃ afɩ i n do? Dɩ tu: Ɩ̃ i n dʋɔn dajɔ gɩdonɩ sɩ jɔrɛ.
41005010	Sɩ a-n phʋʋrɛ Jeju dɩɩ ka ayɩ, a na-n wee kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔlala a faa dɩ khuirə ga.
41005011	Sɩ dabulo sɩthɔ jɔɔ wɛ a kɔɔ hale gɔ̃gɔ̃ khʋra dɩ wa-n khʋʋl.
41005012	Dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiirə phʋʋr Jeju ayɩ: Thɔna sɩ sɩ jal sɩ lõ sɩthɔrara.
41005013	Dɩ ha wɩ hʋɛ wɩ jala, dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔla ther a jal a lõ sɩthɔsɔra bɩnɔ, a tinə wi dɩ wɩ ca birbirbir na gɔ̃gɔ̃ horʋ, a jiir mɩɩr nɔɔra; wɩ kɔɔ daan sɩthɔ gbɩlanɩ yenyɔ a kɔɔ mʋʋlɛ nyʋɔnɔ a khiir.
41005014	Dɩ wɩrɛ n khɛ wɩnɩ, wɩ kɔɔ caar kɔ̃ a mɩɩ dɩɩra na dɩ biisɔra mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛle hanɩ, dɩ tɩbɩla ther jal a hɩɩn mɔ̃ gɩ hanɩ.
41005015	Dɩ wɩ pɔr Jejura a yɩ ʋrɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbii kɔɔ harɔnɩ, kɛ kɔɔ hananɩ dajɔ, dɩ too, a to kɩ̃kɩɩn a hanana dakha yʋ bʋɔ, dɩ maar kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr fɛʋ.
41005016	Wɩrɛ kɔɔ yɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ cʋɛnɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ wɛr gɩrɛ kɔɔ dananɩ ʋrɛ kɔɔ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbii, na gɩrɛ kɔɔ dananɩ sɩthɔsɔ.
41005017	Dɩ le wɩ kɔɔ ma dɩ wa-n phʋʋr Jeju a thɛ wɩ dɩɩra.
41005018	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju n lonɩ gboroona, kuunile kɔɔ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbii phʋʋrʋʋrɛ a dɔ ɩnɩ-n do ɔɔ totoo.
41005019	Sɩ Jeju bor sa sʋʋraa: Kɔna afɩ cɔ afɩ too thɩ̃thɩɩn, a mɩɛnɛ wɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ cʋʋ farnɩ, na mɔ̃ a kɔɔ jɩ fɩnɩ bʋɔra.
41005020	Dɩ mɛ̃ a kɔɔ jal a be da-n wɩɛl paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Dekapol gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Jeju kɔɔ cʋʋraanɩ, dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
41005021	Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ bire iir na gborõo gɩ̃ iiro, dɩ tibil jɔ bir gbɛbɩ wo a pʋɔraa, sɩ mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔra a kɔɔ ha.
41005022	Dɩ kuunikɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jaɩrʋsɩ, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ kɔ̃tɩn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, pɔr a yɩɩ a jiirəə ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn,
41005023	sɩ da-n phʋʋrʋʋ ayɩ: Gɩ-n khor ɩ̃ bikhɛr bu da-n ɓɔr; ɩna dɛɛnaa nyɛ̃ɛ a tagaa a le.
41005024	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju na kuunile jal kha, sɩ tibil jɔ hiirəəre a thʋ̃ dɩ wa-n cʋɔrʋʋ mɔ̃ wɩ-n jalnɩ.
41005025	Dɩ khɛ bɩɛl gɩ, a hale a hana tɩ̃ɩ a cʋʋna yɛna yʋɔr yenyɔ.
41005026	A kɔɔ gaarɛ bʋɔ jɔɔ ka thɩdara jɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ a kʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a hananɩ, sɩrakɛ ga-n haaraa kpɩa', sɩɩ do gɩ ka dɩ a-n dɛbɩrɔrɛ;
41005027	dɩ a sor na ɔɔ bɩ̃: A mɩ puno a thar ɔɔ kẽkenanakɛ dɩbara, ma kpɛɛrɛ.
41005028	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ a-n kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ Jejuuda, a pɔr a 'lɔɔ tibil jɔraale thɩ̃thɩɩn Jejuu khiro a thaaraa kɩ̃kɩɩnna.
41005029	Dɩ dapaara ɔɔ tɔmɩ̃ theele kur, dɩ jɩ ɔɔ tomɩra tue dɩɩ do a kpɛɛrɛ.
41005030	Dɩ le Jeju jɩ na ɔɔ ha dɩ fãga the narɛ gbe, a kɩɩl a bule: Amɛ thaan mar kɩ̃kɩɩnna?
41005031	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara sʋʋraa: Fe yɩ tibil jɔ dɩ wɩ hi far thakɛ sɩ dɩ fɩ yɩ, amɛ thaan farɩ?
41005032	Sɩ Jeju borrakɛ sa hɩɩn da-n finə ɩnɩ-n jɩ ntɛ cʋɛnɩ thalera.
41005033	Dɩ maar fʋ khɛr da-n jẽ a jɩnɩ gɩrɛ danaanɩ, a pɔr a ji Jejuu ƴɛra sa sʋʋraa casɩ mɔ̃ gɩ haaraanɩ.
41005034	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Ɩ̃ bikhɛr afɩ ha pɛ taa fɩ, kɔna na ha ɩɩ a tɔɔna tomɩ kheu.
41005035	Mɔ̃ a hanɩ mɩɩrɔ, tɩbɩla ther Jaɩrʋsɩ kɔ̃tɩnɩ cɔ a pɔ a so: Afɩ bikhɛr khire, anye fɩ-n vɔɔrɔ Dɩɩrdaar 'lo?
41005036	Sɩ Jeju na therna gɩrɛ wɩ sona', sɩ a sor Jaɩrʋsɩra: Fa-n do haar n ubi fa', pɩɛr haar dɩbara.
41005037	Sɩ Jeju na tu tibil bɩɛl n ɩhɔaa saagado Pɩɛr na Jakɩ na Jã, Jakɩɩ õkuunna gaaga.
41005038	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ kɔɔ dã Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩnɩ pa, dɩ Jeju yɩ mɔ̃ khʋ̃ɛ hanɩ, a yɩna tɩbɩla dɩ wa-n bɩ dɩ wa-n bena hulẽbi khena;
41005039	dɩ a lʋʋn sa so war: Anye nɩ-n khʋɔn thakɛ, dɩ anye nɩ-n bɩrɔ, bɩsaanɩkɛ na khə', a-n daarɛ.
41005040	Sɩ wɩ-n maanʋʋnɛ, dɩ agɩpɩ a tire tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩ wɩ thɩɩr, sɩ dɩ kpa bɩsaanɩlee thɩ na nɩrɛ, na wɩrɛ kɔɔ thɔgɔɔnɩ dɩ wɩ lõ ka bɩsaan hanɩ,
41005041	dɩ fʋʋ nyɔ̃ɔ sa sʋʋraa: Talɩta kumɩ; kɩrʋ dʋɔn: Khebir, mɩ so farɛ pala ɩrɛ.
41005042	Dɩ dapaara khebir pal ɩɩr a ma da-n sa, gɩdonɩ a hananɛ yɛna yʋɔr yenyɔ; dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
41005043	Sɩ Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ na sobɔr dɩ wa-n do tibil n jɩ thɩ̃ɛɛla', sɩ a sor wɩ hana khebirile dɩkor a kho.
41006001	Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ ther le a jal ɔɔ dʋɔ, dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ thɔgʋʋrɛ.
41006002	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ hɩɩr wire kɔɔ danɩ, a kɔɔ mar da-n dɩɩr wɩ thɩ̃ɛ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra; dɩ nʋɔ kpaa tibil jɔɔkɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ dɩ wa-n so: Ka a yɩ ga thɩ̃ casɔɔkɛ? Anyee kpɛsɛ ca ha gɩrɛ a hananɩ? Dɩ mɔ̃ a fʋ sɩ da-n cʋʋ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ ca gɩrɛ?
41006003	Ga do thɩ̃ khaadaar gɩ, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ Marɩɩ bikuunaa? Ga do Jakɩ, na Jojɩ, na Juudi, na Sɩmɔ̃ɔ õkuun a doaa? Dɩ ɔɔ õkhɛrsɔ na ha kha kɛ na sɛrɛaa? Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ-n beesuu.
41006004	Sɩ Jeju so warɛ: Wɩ-n cʋrɛ Thãgbaa bobon paar fɛʋ, sɩ ɔɔ dʋɔ na ɔɔ too thɩ̃thɩɩn na ɔɔ cɔ, wa-n cʋa'.
41006005	Dɩ Jeju na-n puno dɩ cʋʋ le nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ bɩɛl, saagado ɩkhaa khodaarsɔ gbe a-n dɛɛnɔ nyɛ̃ɛ dɩ wɩ kpɛaa ga.
41006006	Nʋɔ kɔɔ kpagʋʋrɛ gɩdonɩ wa-n pɩɛ haara'. Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ kpaarɛ le dɩ khuirəsɔ da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ.
41006007	Sɩ agɩpɩ, dɩ we yʋɔr yenyɔ, a ma da-n thɔ̃ wɩ yenyɔ yenyɔ, a ha wɩ punone kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔlala.
41006008	Sɩ a so warɛ, wa-n gba thɩ̃ɛ fʋrɔ jalna kpaar paar saagado gbʋʋl dɩbara gaaga; ayɩ, wa-n fʋrɔ buruə', wa-n fʋrɔ kpakpaar lokaara', wa-n fʋrɔ war pɔtɩmana ga,
41006009	sɩ wɩ tɔ nɛfaa sɩ wa-n to kẽkena yenyɔa'.
41006010	Sɩ dɩ so war: Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ lonɩ cɔ bɩɛlla, nɩ tɔɔ le gɩ dana wireekɛ na thenɩ pa dɔɔle.
41006011	Sɩ ado paar hale kãkɛ tɩbɩla na tee nɩna', wa-n pɛ nɩ dakha nũə', nɩ thɛ pa dɔɔle sa kpɛɛnɛ thɩlãkobeekɛ ma nɩnɩ nɛɛ a faa war, gɩ nɩna wɩ thɩmɩɩr.
41006012	Dɩ kpãkpãadara jaal dɩ wa-n so war wa-n deba haar,
41006013	dɩ wɩ-n weenanɛ dakha kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ jɔɔ dɩ wa-n faa, sɩ dɩ wɩ pɛr khodara jɔɔ niin dɩ wa-n kpɛɛ.
41006014	Dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar nɩɛrɛ gɩdonɩ Jejuu i kpaarɛ paar fɛʋ, dɩ wɩ so ayɩ: Jã Batɩsɩtɩ gɩ, ɔr ɩrɛ khirera, gɛr gɩ dɩ puno da-n cʋʋ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛle.
41006015	Ɩkhasɔ n yɩ wo: Elɩ gɩ; wɛ n yɩ: Thãgbaa bobon gɩ mɔ̃kɛ mamadara kɔɔ hanɩ.
41006016	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ nɩɛnɩ a sor: Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩkɛ mɩ kɔɔ kʋnɩ a kur yʋʋ gɩ, ɔr ɩrɛ khirera.
41006017	Gɩdonɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ thɛthɛ yɩ wɩ fɔ Jã a le tɔ khaɩra. A cʋʋrɛ thale gɩ da Ɛrɔdɩadɩraakɛ dʋɔnnɩ ɔɔ õkuun Filipii khɛr a taanɩ a he;
41006018	dɩ Jã sʋʋraa ga teena a taa ɔɔ õkuuni khɛr a hea'.
41006019	Gɛr hɩna dɩ Ɛrɔdɩadɩ pɛ Jã bɩnɔ da-n ƴaal a kʋʋ, sɩɩ do aa-n mara'.
41006020	Gɩdonɩ maar n fʋrɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ Jana, gɩdonɩ a jɩrɛ dɩɩ do tɩɩ sarʋ gɩ na tɩɩ phuu, dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ na-n ƴaal Jã n yɛ puurə'; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n nɩɛnɩ Jãa thɩmɩɩ kpɩɛrɛ nyanyaanɛ, sɩrakɛ gɩ-n daaraarɛ da-n pɩɛ nũu.
41006021	Sɩ ga kpaanɛ waa dɩɩ do wireekɛ wa jɩnanɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ kɔ̃ wi daan; dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ cʋʋ dɩkɔ jɔɔ, a wena ɔɔ khukhusɔ na sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋsɔ na kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔkɛ hanɩ Galile.
41006022	Dɩ le Ɛrɔdɩadɩɩ bikhɛr lõ ka wɩ hanɩ da-n sa bɩna, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ dar Ɛrɔɔdɩra na wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hanaanɩ kha; dɩ mɛ̃ a so khebirrə: Bɩɛlnɛ mar gɩrɛ fɩ-n ƴaalnɩ dɩ ma ha fɛr;
41006023	dɩ thakɛ a ʋlfɛnaa ayɩ: Ma ha fɛr thɩ̃ dookɛ fa bɩɛl marnɩ, adorakɛ ɩ̃ fãga dɩ kho bɩɛl gɩ.
41006024	Dɩ mɛ̃ khebir the a bule ɔɔ nɩ ayɩ: Ɩ̃ bɩɛlnɛ anye? Dɩ ɔɔ nɩ tu: Bɩɛlnɛ a ha fɩ Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ yʋ.
41006025	Dɩ mɛ̃ khebir phana a kɛr bir fãgadaarɩ pa a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Mɩ-n ƴaalɛ kɔrɔ fɩ pɛ mɩ Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ yʋ kpɛ̃kpɛrɛ̃ biro.
41006026	Dɩ haar n helle Ɛrɔɔdɩ, sɩ aa-n ƴaal a tʋ̃ɔa', gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛnaanɛ dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ kha nɩɛ.
41006027	Dɩ mɛ̃ a thɔ̃ dapaara ɔɔ gardɩ bɩɛl ayɩ, a jala a kuro Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ yʋ a pɔna.
41006028	Dɩ gardɩ kuun jal khaɩra, a kur Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ yʋ, a pɛr kpɛ̃kpɛrɛ̃ biro, a pɔna ha khebir, dɩ khebir gba jalna ha ɔɔ nɩ.
41006029	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jãa kpãkpãadara nɩɛnɩ, wɩ pɔr gba khire a dʋ.
41006030	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔna gbɛbɩ kha na Jeju a mɩɛɛ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ, na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla.
41006031	Dɩ so war: Nɩ dɔ sɩ jal dɩkhãa pa bəənnə nɩ hɩɩr gbe, gɩdonɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ n pɔnɩ Jejura sɩ wa-n kɔ̃ kɔɔ jɔrɛ dɩɩ pho ka, dɩ a do thɔ̃thɔna na ba yɩrɛ ƴɩɛrakɛ na kho dɩkora'.
41006032	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ kɔɔ lõ gborõo a jal paarɩkɛ tibil na hana'.
41006033	Dɩ tibil jɔ yɩ wɛr mɔ̃ wɩ-n jalnɩ a jɩ wɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ the dɩɩsɔra fɛʋ a pɛr nɛpɛla a ka kɔɔ dã paarɩle ɓo.
41006034	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju na thenɩ gboroona, a yɩrɛ tɩbɩlaale tə̃tə̃tə̃ dɩ wa-n kʋʋ bʋɔ, gɩdonɩ wɩ hʋrɛ banasɔɔkɛ na hananɩ khekha', dɩ mɛ̃ a kɔɔ ma da-n dɩɩr wɩ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ.
41006035	Dɩ gɩdonɩ bɔɔ 'lire kar, ɔɔ kpãkpãadara pʋɔraarɛ a sʋʋraa: Dɩɩ n tɩnɛ sɩɩ do bəənnə sɩ ha;
41006036	bɩlanɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ wɩ jal kõgososɔra na dɩ biisɔraakɛ wɔrɔnɛnɩ, wɩ the dɩkɔ.
41006037	Sɩ Jeju tu: Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n hana wɩ dɩkɔ wɩ kho. Sɩ dɩ wɩ bulee: Fɩ-n ƴaalɛ sɩ gba wire taanyɔ thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ war a thɛna buru a ɛna ha wɩ wɩ kho ya?
41006038	Dɩ Jeju bule wi: Buru yemɔ̃ nɩ hana, nɩ jala hɩnɛ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ jɩnɩ tue wɩ sʋʋraarɛ: Buru yemɔɩ sɩ hana na thʋma yenyɔ.
41006039	Agɩpɩ Jeju so war, wɩ cʋɛ tɩbɩlaalera fɛʋ wɩ der dɩɩdɩɩ ka hʋɔn hanɩ vʋɔlvʋɔl.
41006040	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ der tamaa tamaa, kpalanyɔ yʋɔr yʋɔr.
41006041	Agɩpɩ Jeju gba buru yemɔɩɩle na thʋma yenyɔɔle, a gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ a fʋɔr Thãgba, sa kuur buru a ha kpãkpãadara wɩ gba tɩnɛnɛ tɩbɩlala, a tɩnɛna wɩ dakha fɛʋ thʋma yenyɔɔle.
41006042	Wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ khor a hi phi.
41006043	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ gbaar buru na thʋmaakɛ wɩ tɩnɛnɩ sa sɩ dɩɩ hi kpona yʋɔr yenyɔ.
41006044	Sɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ khɔnɩ dɩkorɩle kona daan gbɩlanɩ yemɔɩ.
41006045	Sɩ agɩpɩ, dapaara Jeju yɩ, ɩnɩ kpãkpãadara na lʋʋn gboroona wɩ kʋʋl nɩ ƴɩɛ wɩ iir iiro Bɛcaɩda dɩ khʋra, bɔɔkɛ ɩna-n bɩlanɩ tɩbɩla.
41006046	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ fʋɔr wɩnɩ pɩ sa yɩ wɩ jala bɔɔ, a jaal a jʋʋn gɔ̃gʋɔna a bɩɛl Thãgba.
41006047	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ birəni, gborõo kɔɔ har mɩɩr nɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn, sɩ dɩ Jeju ha dɩbara thɩɩra.
41006048	Dɩ a yɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ phɛllɛ n nɩnɩ kpãkpãadara gɩdonɩ jɩɛ wɩ telẽ, sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ n lɔrnɩ wɩllɛ, a ɩɩrɛ mɩɩr nɔ nyʋɔnna ƴũ da-n pɔ war ɩnɩ-n ka wɩra.
41006049	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ da-n ɩɩr nyʋɔnna ƴũ, wɩ ka jɩna khĩdidaar gɩ, a ma dɩ wa-n hulẽ;
41006050	gɩdonɩ wɛr fɛʋ yɩɩrɛ dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ dɩɩ ka. Sɩ dapaara Jeju mɩɩna wɛr ayɩ: Nɩ pɩɛr 'lar, mɛr Jeju gɩ, na-n do maar n fʋ na'.
41006051	Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ lõ war le gboroona, dɩ jɩɛ kur, dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa kpãkpãadara dɩɩ pho ka,
41006052	gɩdonɩ wa kɔɔ jɩ mɔ̃ buru thɩmɩɩrɩle donɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ kɩrʋa', dəbire gɩ ho war dɩ wa pər gara'.
41006053	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ iirni iiro pɩ a dã Jenejarɛtɩ khʋra, le wɩ kɔɔ li gborõo.
41006054	Dɩ dabɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ thenɩ gboroona na pɩ, dapaara tɩbɩla jɩrɛ Jeju.
41006055	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ ca jal paar fɛʋ a gba khodara jɔna, dɩ wa-n pɔnanaa paar wo paar fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ a har.
41006056	Dɩ paar fɛʋʋkɛ Jeju n jalnɩ, a dɩ biisɔra gɩ, ado dɩɩsɔra gɩ, a kõgoso gɩrakɛ, tɩbɩla n gbaar awɩ khodaarsɔ dɩ wɩ pɛ ƴatɔɔ, dɩ wa-n phʋʋrʋʋ a dɔ ɩna-n thaaraa ɔɔ kẽkẽ nɔra dɩbararakɛ, dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n kɔɔ thaaraanɩ n kpɛɛrɛ awɩ kho.
41007001	Jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na ɩkhaa jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Jerujalɛm pɔr a khunə Jeju;
41007002	dɩ wɩ yɩrɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadaar ɩkhasɔ dɩ wa-n kho dɩkor na nyɛ̃ bise, a thɩɛna gaa nyɛ̃ɛkɛ wa phʋɔlnaa gɩ.
41007003	Gɩdonɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na wɩ̃ Juifisɔ fɛʋ n cʋʋrɛ mɔ̃ awɩ mama kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔ dɩɩr n sonɩ, wa puno na kho dɩkor sɩ a wa kɔɔ jɩɩ hul nyɛ̃aa ga.
41007004	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n thenɩ ƴaa, a wa kɔɔ phʋɔl awɩbara na nyʋɔn ɓoa', wa-n kho dɩkora'. Wɩ hananɛ dakha gɩ̃ mama sosɔɔkɛ wɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ, gɛr dʋɔn thɩ̃ yɔnada cɔcɔɔrɛ, na da cɔcɔɔrɛ, na the bʋla cɔcɔɔrɛ.
41007005	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara bule Jeju: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ afɩ kpãkpãadara na-n gba asɩ mama kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ soa', sɩ dɩ wa-n kho dɩkor na nyɛ̃ bise?
41007006	Dɩ Jeju tu: Sobɔr Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩ kɔɔ so anɩdara ger waa: Bɩnɛ yenyɔdara ha nɩ, gɩdonɩ mɛ̃ gɩ khere mɔ̃ Thãgba sonɩ ayɩ: “Nɔfaar tibil ca ƴɩrɛ n cʋna mɩ pɔɩ, sɩ dɩ awɩ ha hʋnɔna mɩ fĩi.
41007007	Fʋɔrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n fʋɔr mɩnɩ, mɔlɔ gɩ, gɩdonɩ jɔfʋʋkɛ tɩbɩla pɛrnɩ wɩ-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla.”
41007008	Nɩ faarɛ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ sɩ dɩ na-n dʋ mama kɔ̃tɩnaa sora bʋrɛ.
41007009	Sɩ Jeju bir so war: Nɩ jɩrɛ gbobi sa hɛbɩ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ a faa, sɩ dɩ nɩ ka na ɔ mama kɔ̃tɩnaa sora.
41007010	Gɩdonɩ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sor ayɩ: “Na cɔ afɩ thɩ na afɩ nɩ” dɩ “a ntɛ nɩɩr ɔɔ thɩ, a ɔɔ nɩ gɩ, wɩ kʋɔ.”
41007011	Sɩ dɩ ner n so: Ado tibil so ɔɔ ɩhɩra a ɔɔ nɩra gɩ ayɩ: Thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ ma kɔɔ ha fɩnɩna gɩ bul fi, gɛr mɩ gba dɩɩ do Kɔrbã, a thɩɛna gaa, gɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaada;
41007012	mɛ̃ na-n haa hʋɛ a bul ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ bã.
41007013	Mɛ̃ anɩ mama kɔ̃tɩnaa sookɛ nɩ-n kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl cʋʋ Thãgbaa so dɩ ga do thɩ̃ɛ bã. Yɛ̃ thɩ̃sɔ hale wo jɔɔ nɩ-n ɓaannɩ dɩ a-n ho kha na gɩrɛra.
41007014	Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ bire we tibil jɔ dɩ wɩ pɔ dɩ so war: Nɛrɛ fɛʋ nɩ pɛ mɩ nũu a jɛ mɔ̃ gɩ hanɩ.
41007015	Thɩ̃ɛ na hakɛ jɩɛra na lõ tibili bɩnɔ na cʋgʋʋ da bisə', sɩ gɩrɛ n kanɩ dɩɩ the tibili hara gɛr n bisene tibil.
41007016	[Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a pɛ nũu.]
41007017	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ faanɩ tibil jɔɔle sa lõ cʋɔrɔ, ɔɔ kpãkpãadara buleele sokpaalee kɩrra.
41007018	Dɩ so war: Nɛrɛ dakha jɩɩr 'lũ ner dakha wo koe. Na jɩ gɩ dɩ a thɩ̃ɛ kɛ jɩɛra lõ tibil bɩnɔ, ga puno na cʋgʋʋ da bisəə gaa?
41007019	Gɩdonɩ ga do haarra gɩ lõa', sɩɩ do bucuurə gɩ-n lõ sɩ dɩɩ the cuu. A sonɩ thale gɛr nɛna dɩ dɩkor na hale na sãsa'.
41007020	Sɩ a bire so wo: Gɩrɛ n thɛnɩ tibili hara n bisenee.
41007021	Gɩdonɩ bɩnɔ, tibil haarra, le kpɩɛr puu n the, na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ, na yuur, na tɩɩ kʋr,
41007022	na khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaalɛ, na kũu kpɩɩ ƴaalɛ, na ha pɩɛrɛ, na kpallɛ, na tɩɩ fɩɩlɛ, na dakhaba cʋʋrɛ, na yir, na tibil i kʋɛrɛ, na i ƴaalɛ, na də̃bəəle.
41007023	Ga thɩ̃ puu ca ƴɩrɛ fɛʋ, tibil haarra gɩ-n the, dɩ gɛr n bisene tibil.
41007024	Agɩpɩ Jeju the le a jal Tɩɩr dɩ khʋra a lõ cɔ bɩɛlla, sɩ aa-n ƴaal tibil n ja'; sɩ aa puno a mar dɩ wa jaa ga.
41007025	Sɩ khɛ bɩɛl gɩ dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl kɔɔ lõ ɔɔ bikhɛr burə; mɔ̃kɛ khɛrɩle nɩɛnɩ Jejuuda, a pɔr a jii ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
41007026	Gɩrɛkɩ khɛrɩle do sa the Siri Fenɩsɩ dɩɩra; a kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ Jeju a wea kɔ̃tɛɛbuu ɩnɩ bikhɛrra a faa.
41007027	Sɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dɔ bɩsana n kɔɔ kho dɩkor ɓo, gɩdonɩ ga bɔr dɩ fa gba bɩsanaa dɩko na pɛ bena ga.
41007028	Dɩ khɛr tu: Sobɔr gɩ wer Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩ dakurusɔɔkɛ bɩsana na-n khonɩ dɩ ga-ɩɩ ji thʋuɔ, bebe n khor.
41007029	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ fɩ tuni thakɛ kɔna, kɔ̃tɛɛbuu ther afɩ bikhɛr burə.
41007030	Dɩ mɛ̃ a kɔ̃ a yɩ ɔɔ bɩsã dɩ phɩ̃, dɩɩ do kɔ̃tɛɛbuu thɩɩraarɛ.
41007031	Agɩpɩ Jeju ther Tɩɩr khʋra, a kpãsɛ Sɩdɔ̃ ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n birni Galile mɩɩr nɔɔra, a kar Dekapol khʋra.
41007032	Dɩ le wɩ kpa kũu nʋʋr bɩɛlɩkɛ na-n punoneni dɩ mɩɩ thɩmɩa bɔɔbɔa', a pɔna a phʋʋrna Jeju, a dɛɛnaa nyɛ̃ɛ.
41007033	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju faa tɩbɩla sa kpaa, a thena khuirə, a gba nyɛ̃be a tʋʋ nũ kanana, sa phii nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ a thananaa delẽbirera.
41007034	Agɩpɩ Jeju gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ a 'wɩɩ sa so kuunna: Efata, kɩrʋ dʋɔn: Khɛra.
41007035	Dɩ dapaara kuuni nũ ka khɛr, dɩ gɩrɛ kɔɔ lieni delẽbire thʋbɩ, dɩ puno da-n mɩɩ thɩmɩɩr dɩ a-n yɩr dɩphã.
41007036	Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ sor tɩbɩlala fɛʋ, dɩ wa-n gba na mɩɩ tibil n nɩa'. Sɩ mɔ̃ a-n jɩɩnɩ kpãkpãa war jɔɔ wa-n mɩa', gɛr wɩ-n ka mɩɩrɔ dɩ a-n jɔr.
41007037	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ tɩbɩla dɩɩ pho ka dɩ wa-n so aa: Thɩ̃ bɔ haar or n cʋʋrakɛ dɩ thʋ̃ dɩ cʋʋ nʋra ɓoɓo dɩ wa-n nɩ na nɔ masɔ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ.
41008001	Ga bɔɔlera tibil jɔ bir gbɛbɩ wo, sɩ wa hana thɩ̃ɛ na khoa'; dɩ Jeju we ɔɔ kpãkpãadara a so war ayɩ:
41008002	Bʋɔ fʋ mɛr tɩbɩlalaakɛ, gɩdonɩ wire yẽther ha gɩrɛ wɩ hanɩ kha na mɛrɛ, sɩ wa hana thɩ̃ɛ na khoa'.
41008003	Ado mɩ bɩlã wɩ wɩ kɔna sɩ dɩ wa yɩ dɩkora', ga khabɩ wɛr hʋɛra, gɩdonɩ ɩkhasɔ wɛrra ther ƴɔɔ.
41008004	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara sʋʋraa: Ka sa puno na yɩ dɩkɔ na ha tibil ca ƴɩrɛ kɩɛr bəənnə dɩ wa hi.
41008005	Dɩ Jeju bule wi: Buru yemɔ̃ nɩ hana? Dɩ wɩ tu: Makonyɔ gɩ.
41008006	Dɩ Jeju so tɩbɩlalaale wɩ dera, sa gba buru makonyɔra a fʋɔr Thãgba pɛr, sa kuur a ha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, wɩ gba tɩnɛnɛ tibil jɔɔlera; dɩ wɩ gba tɩnɛ wɩ.
41008007	Sɩ wɩ hananɛ dakha dɩkhaa thʋ̃ bi, dɩ Jeju fʋɔr Thãgba a pɛr thʋmanaale, sa so wɩ tɩnɛnɛ wɩ dakha.
41008008	Wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ khor a hi phi; dɩ kpãkpãadara gbaar dakurusɔɔkɛ sɛnɩ dɩɩ hi kpona makonyɔ.
41008009	Sɩ konaale kɔɔ thɔɔrɛ gbɩlanɩ yenã. Agɩpɩ Jeju bɩlã wɩ,
41008010	sa lõ dapaara gboroona na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara a jal Dalmanuta khʋra.
41008011	Jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara wɛ, a pɔ a ma dɩ wa-n bana kha na Jeju wɩ pɩɛraa pheru, a bulee ayɩ, a nɛ nar na nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ bɩɛl dɩ ɔɔ punona thãgbara ƴũ gɩ the.
41008012	Dɩ Jeju 'wɩɩ na bɩnɛ sa so: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nĩdara na-n ƴaal nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ ya fɛ? Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wa nɩna wɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ bɩɛllaka'.
41008013	Agɩpɩ dɩ faa wɩ, sa bir lõ gboroona a iir gɩ̃ iiro.
41008014	Sɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ diinəne buru gbaar, sɩɩ do bɩɛl dɩbara wɩ hana le gboroona.
41008015	Dɩ Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ ayɩ: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, na-n tɛ̃tɛna jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ taba'.
