41008016	Dɩ kpãkpãadara na-n mɩɩ kha bururaakɛ wa kɔɔ gbana'.
41008017	Dɩ Jeju jɩ mɔ̃ wɩ-n mɩɩnɩ kha a bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n mɩɩ kha bururaakɛ na kɔɔ gbana? Na yɩ gaa, dɩ na jɩ kɩrʋ paa? Anɩdara khɩɩrɛ waa gel koe.
41008018	Yinəna nɩ hananɩ wo na-n yaa? A hanana nũu wo na-n naa? Dɩ na jɩna gaa?
41008019	Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ kuurni buru yemɔɩ a ha kona gbɩlanɩ yemɔɩ, kpona yemɔ̃ nɩ kɔɔ gba dakuruukɛ sɛnɩ dɩɩ hi? Dɩ wɩ tu: Kpona yʋɔr yenyɔ gɩ.
41008020	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ kuurni buru makonyɔ a ha kona gbɩlanɩ yenã, kpona yemɔ̃ nɩ kɔɔ gba dakuruukɛ sɛnɩ dɩɩ hi? Dɩ wɩ tu: Makonyɔ gɩ.
41008021	Dɩ Jeju so war: Na yɩ gɩ a thʋ̃ jɩ kɩrʋ pɩrakɛ mãa?
41008022	Wɩ kɔɔ danɩ Bɛcaɩda le tɩbɩla kpa yaarʋ, a pɔna Jejura dɩ wa-n phʋʋrnaa a thaaraa.
41008023	Dɩ Jeju fʋrɛ yaarʋʋle nyɔ̃ɔ, a kpaa thena dɩ khuirə, a phii nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ pɩɛraa yinəna, a dɛɛnanaa nyɛ̃ɛ sa bulee: Fɩ yɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ ya?
41008024	Dɩ yaarʋ gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ sa so: Mɩ yɩrɛ tɩbɩla, sɩ mɩ yɩ wɛr dɩ wɩ ho thɩra dɩ wa-n ɩɩr.
41008025	Sɩ Jeju bir thaaraa yinəna wo, dɩ dabɔɔkɛ yaarʋ kponɩ yinə, dɩɩ do a khɛrrɛ da-n yɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ wawawal.
41008026	Sɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Kɔna, fa-n kɛr bir lõ dɩɩra sa kɔ̃a'.
41008027	Agɩpɩ Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara gba jal Sejare Filipi dɩ khʋra; dɩ le a bule ɔɔ kpãkpãadara hʋɛra: Amɛ tɩbɩla n yɩ mɩ dor?
41008028	Dɩ wɩ tu: Ɩkhasɔ n yɩ, Jã Batɩsɩtɩ fɩ do; wɛ n yɩ, Elɩ fɩ do; wɛ n yɩ wo, Thãgbaa bobon fɩ do.
41008029	Sɩ Jeju bule wi: Sɩ ner, amɛ nɩ-n yɩ mɩ dor? Dɩ Pɩɛr tu: Kirisiti fɩ do.
41008030	Sɩ Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ, wa-n so tibillə ga.
41008031	Agɩpɩ Jeju ma da-n dɩɩr ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, da-n sona war ayɩ: Dɔ mɛrkɛ dʋɔnnɩ tibili Bikuun n gaar bʋɔ jɔɔ; dɩ kɔ̃tɩna, na bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na bo mer, sɩ dakha wa kʋ mɛr, sɩ a wire yẽther ka ma ɩɩrɛ khirera.
41008032	Casɩ a-n mɩɩ wɩ gele. Sɩ Pɩɛr kpaa kana pa kpɩɩ da-n phaan.
41008033	Sɩ Jeju kɛr, da-n hɩɩn ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, sa phã Pɩɛr dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ: Hala mɩ ƴɔɔ Satã, gɩdonɩ fa-n kpɩɛr Thãgbaa kha ga, sɩ tibil khaa fɩ-n kpɩɛr.
41008034	Agɩpɩ Jeju we tibil jɔ na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara dɩ wɩ pʋɔraa dɩ so war: A ntɛ pɛr haar ɩna-n kpa mar, dɔ a faa dɩbara yɩrnanɛ, sɩ a gba ɔɔ kʋkʋ thɩr a na-n kpana mar.
41008035	Gɩdonɩ tibilikɛ n tɛbanɩ ɔɔ yi, ga ka na buurəəre; sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ yi na bonɩ mɛrɛra, na Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra, ɔr na lɛ waa gel.
41008036	Anyee bɔ ga taa tibil, ado a 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ sɩɩ do ɔɔ yi buurəəre.
41008037	Anye haankɛ dɩ tibil na gba na debina ɔɔ yi?
41008038	A yicuru fʋ tibil mɛrɛra na ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩra nĩdaraakɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, kɛ na telenenɩ Thãgbara ga, sɩ dɩ wa-n cʋʋ puure, yicuru na fʋrɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun dakha ntɛra, ɔbɔɔkɛ ma ɩnɩ na ɩ̃ Thɩɩ i dʋbɩ nakha thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu phuusɔ.
41009001	Dɩ so war wo ayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ɩkhasɔɔkɛ hanɩ kɩɛr na khiir sɩɩ do wa yɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do dɩɩ ɩ̃ na fãga gaaga.
41009002	A wire maadõ ka pɩ, Jeju kpar Pɩɛr na Jakɩ na Jã a jʋʋnna gɔ̃gɔ̃ gbaana, dɩ wɩ ha kha le dɩbara; dɩ Jejuu tomɩ debi awɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
41009003	Dɩ ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ debi dɩ a-n hɩl phalphalphal, a bulololakɛ dakha dɩɩ ka, a jɔ mɔ̃kɛ ga donɩ tibil thɩɩraakɛ na punone na cʋʋ dɩ a buloloa'.
41009004	Dɩ Elɩ na Mʋɩjɩ the warɛ sɩ Jeju wɩ-n khʋɛna.
41009005	Dɩ Pɩɛr so Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, gɩ bɔrɛ sɩ hanɩ kɩɛr; sa dʋrɛ waa yẽther, bɩɛl n do afɩda, bɩɛl n do Mʋɩjɩɩda, bɩɛl n do Elɩɩda.
41009006	Aa jɩ mɔ̃ a na sona', gɩdonɩ maar fʋɔn wɛr kpãkpãadara.
41009007	Dɩ ndɔlɔ̃paar gbune a thi war, dɩ nʋɔ the ndɔlɔ̃paarra ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, na-n pɩɛ nũu.
41009008	Dɩ dapaara kpãkpãadara hɩɩnɛ khʋʋkhʋʋ, sɩ wa kɔɔ yɩ tibil saagado Jeju gɩ dɩbara na wɛraa ga.
41009009	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ gbuni gɔ̃gʋɔna, Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ na sobɔr dɩ wa-n so tibillə gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ kɔɔ yɩna', phaphapha ɩnɛr tibili Bikuun n ɩɩr khirera.
41009010	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ thɩmɩɩrɩle awɩ bɩnɔ, sɩ wa-n bule khasɔ aa: Anye n dɔ khi ɩɩrɛ?
41009011	Sɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ buleele thakɛ ayɩ: Mɔ̃ gɩ ha dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na-n so ayɩ: Dɔ Elɩ n kɔɔ ɩ̃ caca.
41009012	Dɩ tu: Elɩ na kɔɔ ɩna wer eaca na wɛbɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ. Sɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩɩ khere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra mɛr tibili Bikuunidara ayɩ: Dɔ ɩ̃ gaar bʋɔ jɔɔ dɩ wa therna ma?
41009013	Sɩ mɩ so narɛ, Elɩ kɔɔ ɩnɛ sɩ wɩ kɔɔ cʋgʋʋrɛ mɔ̃ wɩ pɛrnɩ haar, dɩɩ ha mɔna gɩ kɔɔ khereraanɩ.
41009014	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ danɩ wɩ̃ kpãkpãadara, wɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ tibil jɔ dɩ wɩ dii war na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔɔkɛ n bananɛnanɩ kpãkpãadaraale thɩ̃ banaa.
41009015	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil jɔɔle yɩnɩ Jeju, gɩ phuro wer dɩ wɩ ca pɔ a fʋɔrʋʋ.
41009016	Dɩ bule wi: Anye nɩ-n bana kha na wɛr?
41009017	Dɩ kũu bɩɛl tibil jɔraale tu: Dɩɩrdaar, mɩ kɔɔ kpar ɩ̃ bikuunikɛ hananɩ nɔ ma kɔ̃tɛɛbuu a ɩna far;
41009018	pa dɔɔkɛ a-n fʋʋnɩ thɩɩra a-n kpɛgʋʋ, dɩ bɩsaan na-n the nyɔ̃thɩ̃ khɔrɔ̃ɔ, da-n khona nyɩma, sɩ dɩ tã gõgorõo; dɩ mɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ afɩ kpãkpãadara wɩ wea kɔ̃tɛɛbuurə, sɩ wa kɔɔ punoə'.
41009019	Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɛr nĩ babalaakɛɛ; ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ma thʋ̃ na toona nɩ gɩ dana? Ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ma thʋ̃ na fʋ nar haarrarakɛ gɩ dana? Nɩ kpaa ɛna mar.
41009020	Dɩ wɩ kpaa a pɔna; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuu na yɩnɩ Jeju, a gbʋ̃gbʋnyanɛ bɩsaan dɩ ji thʋnɔ da-n laan, da-n thena nyɔ̃thɩ̃ khɔrɔ̃ɔ.
41009021	Dɩ Jeju bule thɩrɛ: A fʋna ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔrakɛ gekɛra wer kɔɔ hanaa? Dɩ thɩrɛ tu: Ɔɔ bɩsã bu bɔɔ gɩ.
41009022	Dɩ wire wire kɔ̃tɛɛbuule n tʋɔrɛ da-n kpɛɛ dɔɔ na nyʋɔnɔ ɩnɩ-n kʋʋra; sɩ ado fa punone na cʋʋ dɩkha, jɛ sɩ bʋɔra sa bulo si.
41009023	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Fɩ yɩ, ado ma punone ya? Thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ n punone ʋrɛraakɛ pɩɛrnɩ Thãgba haar.
41009024	Dapaara bɩsaanɩlee thɩ hulẽ ayɩ: Mɩ pɛrɛ haar, bulo mi ɩ̃ baallala.
41009025	Mɔ̃ Jeju yɩnɩ tɩbɩla dɩ wɩ ca pɔ wa-n jɔr, le a mana kɔ̃tɛɛbuu ayɩ: Fɛr nʋʋr nɔ ma kɔ̃tɛɛbuu, mɛr sɔ far: A fɩ jɩ thɛ bɩsaannaakɛ, fa-n lʋʋnaa yuu bã.
41009026	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ a-n thenɩ a hulene sa gbʋ̃gbʋnyã bɩsaan na fãga, dɩ bɩsaan debi a ho a khire pɔɩ; wɩrɛ wer hanɩlerakɛ yɩ: A khire.
41009027	Sɩ Jeju fʋʋ nyɔ̃ɔ a khəi dɩ pal ɩɩr.
41009028	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju lonɩ cʋɔrɔ dɩ wɩ ha kha na kpãkpãadara dɩbara, wɩ buleele aa: Mɔ̃ gɩ fʋna dɩ ser na kɔɔ puno a wee kɔ̃tɛɛbuule a fa ga?
41009029	Dɩ so war: Agado Thãgba bɩɛlɛ ga, kɔ̃tɛɛbu ca ʋrɛ na hana ther na tha'.
41009030	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ ther le a jal a kpãsɛ Galile, sɩ Jeju na kɔɔ ƴaal wɩ jɛ ka a hana';
41009031	gɩdonɩ a-n dɩɩrɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, da-n sona war ayɩ, wa fʋrɛ ɩnɛrkɛ dɔnɩ tibili Bikuun na ha tɩbɩla dɩ wa kʋ nɩ, sɩ a ɩnɩ khi dɩ wire yẽther ka, ɩna ɩɩrɛ khirera.
41009032	Sɩ kpãkpãadara na jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩle kɩrʋa', dɩ maar kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr dɩ wa 'la na bulea'.
41009033	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan Kapɛrnayʋm; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ hanɩ cʋɔrɔ, gɛr Jeju bulelo ɔɔ kpãkpãadara ayɩ: Anye nɩ-n kɔɔ bana kha hʋɛrara?
41009034	Dɩ wɩ pɩr pɔɔpɔɔ, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ jɩ ʋrɛ 'lɛnɩ kɔ̃tɩɩnɛ, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ kɔɔ bana kha hʋɛra.
41009035	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju too sa we kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ, dɩ wɩ pɔ dɩ so war ayɩ: Ntɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩnɩ-n dɔ ƴɛ kʋl, dɔ a do pɩpɩr tɩbɩlala fɛʋ na tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ thɔ̃daar.
41009036	Agɩpɩ dɩ kpa bɩsã buu a pɔna awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, sa gbaa fʋrɔ sa so war:
41009037	Ntɛɛkɛ na teanɩ bɩsaan thakɛ a na-n hɩɩn, gɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ, mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ a tee. Dɩ ntɛɛkɛ tea mɩnɩ, ga do mɛr a tea', sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ a tee.
41009038	Jã so Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ tibilikɛ na dɔnɩ asɩ kpakpaara', dɩ gba afɩ i dɩ weena kɔ̃tɛɛbii da-n faa, dɩ sa-n kɔɔ pɩɛrʋʋ gɩdonɩ aa do asɩ kpakpaara'.
41009039	Dɩ Jeju tu: Na-n ha na pɩɛrʋa', gɩdonɩ tibil na puno na gba ɩ̃ i na cʋʋna nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ, saa kɛr dapaara wo a mɩɩ ɩ̃da puə'.
41009040	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n ƴaalɛ sɩnɩ sʋa', sɛrra a-n pɛ.
41009041	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ ɩ̃ i na donɩ nɔɔ dɩ na cɛ nyʋɔn na ha nɩ nɩ yɔ, gɩdonɩ Kirisitii too nɩ do, sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, thɩ̃ɛ na hale na pɩɛrʋʋ lɩmɩ 'lɛrra ga.
41009042	Nã kɔ̃tɩ̃ tə̃ə lir tibillə fʋɔrɔ wɩ dʋnanaa lanyʋɔnɔ, baar gɩrɛɛkɛ a na kanɩ na cʋʋ dɩ bɩsã biikɛ pɛ mɩnɩ haar dɩ bɩɛl na bara.
41009043	Ado afɩ nyɔ̃ do far baradaa, kuro faa. A fɩ 'lɛ yire na nyɔ̃ bɩɛl, gɩ baar nyɛ̃ɛ yenyɔɔkɛ fa hananɩ sɩ wɩ dʋna fɩ bu paar dɔɔraakɛ na dɔnɩ thɩ̃ khiirnənə'.
41009044	[Le dɔ na-n khə', dɩ dɔɔ dakha na-n khiir kpɩɩa'.]
41009045	Ado afɩ nɔ do far baradaa, kuro faa. A fɩ 'lɛ yire na nɔ bɩɛl, gɩ baar nɛɛ yenyɔɔkɛ fa hananɩ sɩ wɩ dʋna fɩ bu paar dɔɔra.
41009046	[Le dɔ na-n khə', dɩ dɔɔ dakha na-n khiir kpɩɩa'.]
41009047	Ado afɩ yi do far baradaa, te faa. A fɩ lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dʋɔ na yi khoroo, gɩ baar yinə yenyɔɔkɛ fa hananɩ sɩ wɩ dʋna fɩ bu paar dɔɔra.
41009048	Le dɔ na-n khə', dɩ dɔɔ dakha na-n khiir kpɩɩa'.
41009049	Gɩdonɩ dɔɔ na cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ ga hana laanɩ mɩla.
41009050	Thɩ̃ bʋɔ laan do, sɩ a laan bir dasɩ a mɩla bã, mɔ̃ wa fʋ sɩ na cʋʋ dɩ a bir na hana mɩlalɛ?
41009051	Nɩ hanana laan anɩ bɩnɔ, dɩ nɩ hanana kha ha ɩɩ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
41010001	Jeju ther le a gba jal Jude khʋra, sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ ɩɩr Jʋrdɛ̃ iiro. Dɩ tibil jɔ n gbɛbɩ dɩ wɩ pɔ na derraa, dɩ ma da-n dɩɩr wɩ thɩ̃ɛ mɔ̃ a mɩlna gɩnɩ.
41010002	Ɩkhaa jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara pʋɔraarɛ, dɩ wa-n fifiləə a bulee thakɛ ayɩ: Tibil hananɛ hʋɛ na faa ɔɔ khɛr ya?
41010003	Dɩ tu: Anyee jɔfʋ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ ha nɩ?
41010004	Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa ayɩ: Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ 'laarɛ hʋɛ, kuun n khera he kuur sɛbɛ sa wea ɔɔ khɛr a faa.
41010005	Dɩ Jeju so war: Anɩdara khiinoni dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ khere nar jɔfʋ caale.
41010006	Sɩ fʋ paar, ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ tini thɩ̃ɛ, kuun na khɛr a kɔɔ cʋʋ.
41010007	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ kuun na lee kha na ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ, sɩ a ɓã kha na ɔɔ khɛr,
41010008	wɛr yenyɔ n gbɛbɩ wɩ do tibil bɩɛl, mɛ̃ ga do yenyɔ ha bã, sɩ wɩ coore kha a do bɩɛl.
41010009	Gɛr gɩ ga teena tibil n lea gɩrɛ Thãgba coornɩ dɩɩ do bɩɛla'.
41010010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ hanɩ cʋɔrɔ, kpãkpãadara bire bule Jeju ga so caalera,
41010011	dɩ so war: A tibil faa ɔɔ khɛr sa bir a he khɛ kpɩɩ, khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaal sopugo a cʋʋ ɔɔ caca khɛrra.
41010012	Ado khɛr gɩ a faa ɔɔ ko sa bir he kũu kpɩɩ, kũu kpɩɩ ƴaal sopugo a cʋʋ.
41010013	Dɩ tɩbɩla kɔɔ kpar bɩsana a pɔna Jejura, a dɛɛnɛ war nyɛ̃ɛ, sɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ phaanɛ wɩrɛ pɔna wɩnɩ.
41010014	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju yɩɛnɩ nĩkhii fʋʋrɛ, dɩ so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Nɩ dɔ bɩsana na-n ɩ̃ mar, na-n pɩɛr wa', gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ hɔnɩ bɩsana, wɛr Thãgbaa fãgadaar do mana.
41010015	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n tuonni Thãgbaa fãgadaar do bɩsanaa khaaka', a na puno na lono kpɩɩraka'.
41010016	Agɩpɩ dɩ gba bɩsana a fʋrɔ, sa dɛ̃ɛ war fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl nyɛ̃ɛ a bɔna wɩ.
41010017	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju n gbanɩ hʋɛ, kũu bɩɛl car pʋɔraa a gulẽgaraa a bulee: Dɩɩrdaar bʋɔ, anye ma cʋʋ na 'lɛ yire khorr?
41010018	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fɩ we mɩ dabʋɔ? Tɩɩ bʋɔ na hala', Thãgba dɩbara bʋɔnɔ.
41010019	Fɩ jɩrɛ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ: “Fa-n kʋ tibilə', fa-n hana khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n hana kũu kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n yuə', fa-n sõso pɛ tibilə', fa-n pɛr fɩɩlɛ thɩɛna ga, na cɔ afɩ thɩ na afɩ nɩ.”
41010020	Dɩ kuunile tu: Dɩɩrdaar mɩ kɔɔ mãa nɩ ga jɔfʋraale fɛʋ nũu kɛkɛkɛ ɩ̃ daɓol dĩi bɔɔ.
41010021	Dɩ Jeju hɩɩnʋʋ na naʋ sa sʋʋraa: Thɩ̃ bɩɛl ɓɔr fɛr, jala dolone thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ fɩ hananɩ a hana bɔdara, dɩ mɛ̃ fa 'lɛ lẽle thɩ̃ɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, agɩpɩ fɩ ɩ̃ fa-n kpa mar.
41010022	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ kuunile nɩɛnɩ thɩmɩɩ ca gele a gbure ƴɩɛ, sa gba da-n kɔna gbobire, gɩdonɩ lẽledaar gɩ na sobɔr.
41010023	Sɩ Jeju hɩɩn ɔɔ kpãkpãadara da-n finə sa so war: Thãgba fãgadaar dɩ lʋʋn khɩɩrɛ waa gel wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ lɛ̃lɛ.
41010024	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ kpãkpãadara fɛʋ ga thɩmɩɩ caraale; sɩ Jeju bir so war wo: Ɩ̃ bɩsãsɔ, Thãgba fãgadaar dɩ lʋʋn khɩɩrɛ waa gel.
41010025	Nyɔɔmɛɛ lõokɛ a na lonɩ mɩsɩmɩ kaarra ka yɔɔrɛ jɔ lẽlee Thãgba fãgadaar dɩ lõ.
41010026	Sɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ kpãkpãadara dɩɩ ka thɩmɩɩrraale, dɩ wa-n bule khasɔ bɩɛlbɩɛl aa: Dɩ a mɛ̃ gɩ, amɛ na punone na 'lɛ taarɛ?
41010027	Dɩ Jeju hɩɩn wɩ sa so: Ado tɩbɩlala wer gɩ, thɩ̃ punonaa ga; sɩ ga ha mɛ̃ Thãgbara ga, gɩdonɩ Thãgba n punone thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
41010028	Sɩ Pɩɛr ma da-n sʋʋraa: Hɩnɛ, sɛrɛ sɩ faarɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ sɩ sa-n kpa far.
41010029	Dɩ Jeju tu: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ado tibil faa ɔɔ cɔ, a ɔɔ õkona wɛ, a ɔɔ õkhɛrsɔ wɛ, a ɔɔ nɩ gɩ, a ɔɔ thɩ gɩ, a ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ wɛ, a ɔɔ lɛ gɩ, dɩɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ na Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra,
41010030	a na 'lɛr thɩ̃ɛ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛ tama tama der paar tamaa: Gɔnasɔ, õkonasɔ, õkhɛnasɔ, nɛsɔ, bɩsanasɔ, na lɩɛsɔ, a na 'lɛnanɛ dakha kpoore, sɩ bɔɔkɛ na ɩnanɩ a na 'lɛr yire khorr.
41010031	Sɩ tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ nɛnɛ̃ ƴɛ kʋla, wɛr na fien na do sɩka pɩra, sɩ tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ nɛnɛ̃ sɩka pɩra, wɛr na fien na do ƴɛ kʋla.
41010032	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ gbaar hʋɛ dɩ wa-n jal Jerujalɛm, dɩ Jeju kʋʋl wɩ ƴɩɛ. Sɩ haar fuure kpãkpãadara dɩ maar fʋ dakha wɩrɛ n kpaaraanɩ. Dɩ Jeju bir kpa kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ dɩ wɩ ha kha, dɩ ma da-n mɩɛ wɩ gɩrɛ na danaanɩ.
41010033	A so warɛ ayɩ: Nɩ hɩnɛ, sɩ-n jaal gɩrɛ Jerujalɛm, ka wa fʋnɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na ha bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ, dɩ wa pɛ mar so kʋnanɛ; sɩ na gba mɩ na ha ca kpala;
41010034	dɩ wa mãa mɛr, wɩ cɩɩrna nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ wa-n pɛ mar, wa ciil mer dakha na khasa, sɩ wɩ kʋ mɩ, sɩ a wire yẽther ka ma ɩɩrɛ khirera.
41010035	Agɩpɩ Jebedee bikonaakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jakɩ na Jã pɔ Jejura, a sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar, cʋɛ sar gɩrɛ sa bɩɛl farnɩ.
41010036	Dɩ bule wi: Anye nɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋɛ nar?
41010037	Dɩ wɩ tu: A fɩ gba afɩ fãga, ha sɩ hʋɛ, bɩɛl n too afɩ nyɔ̃bɔra, bɩɛl afɩ nyɔ̃bɩlana.
41010038	Sɩ Jeju so war: Na jɩ gɩrɛ nɩ-n bɩɛlna'; na punone na yɔ thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ bɔ gaarɛɛkɛ ma yɔnɩ ya? Agɩbo wɩ kpɛɛ nɩ bɔ gaarɛraakɛ wa kpɛɛ mɩnɩ yɔ khaa ya?
41010039	Dɩ wɩ tu: Ɔɔ, sa punone. Dɩ Jeju so war: Sobɔr gɩ, thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ ma yɔnɩ na yɔr, dɩ yɔ kpɛɛrɛɛkɛ ma 'lɛnɩ na 'lɛr dakha.
41010040	Sɩ ga do mɛr na phire ʋrɛ na tɔɔnɩ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra na ʋrɛ na tɔɔnɩ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɩlana ga; wɩrɛ dɩbara Thãgba gbɛbɩrɔnɩ too paa caarɩkɛ, awɩda gɩ.
41010041	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ gele, nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋ wɛr Jakɩra na Jã.
41010042	Dɩ Jeju we wɩ dɩ wɩ pɔ, dɩ so war: Nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ wɩrɛ wɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ dɩ wɛr dɔ ca kpalaa fãgadara, wɩ-n ʋʋnɛ tɩbɩlala kpɛ, dɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩna n cʋʋ warɛ fãga dɩɩ pho ka.
41010043	Sɩ ga ha mɛ̃ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩna', sɩ ntɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩnɩ-n dɔ kɔ̃tɩn, dɔ ɔr n ka a do anɩ thɔ̃daar.
41010044	Ado tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra ƴaal ɩnɩ-n dɔ ƴɛ kʋl, dɔ ɔr n do tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ dee.
41010045	Gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na ɩ̃ tibil na-n dɔ mar thɔma ga, sɩ mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ ka ɩ̃ do thɔma sɩ ɩ̃ 'laa ɩ̃ yi gɩ birse tɩbɩla bərəəm.
41010046	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan Jeriko; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara na tibil jɔ na ɩɩrnɩ dɩɩraale na the, bɛ̃bɩɛl yaarʋʋkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Bartɩme, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ Timee bikuun, kɔɔ toore le hʋ nʋɔra.
41010047	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a nɩɛnɩ dɩ Najarɛtɩ Jeju n pʋɔn, a mar da-n hulẽ aa: Jeju Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun, jɛ mɩ bʋɔra.
41010048	Sɩ tibil jɔ kɔɔ manaanɛ ayɩ a pɩra; sɩ a ka jɩɛ bir hulẽ wo aa: Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun, jɛ mɩ bʋɔra.
41010049	Dɩ Jeju jɩɩl sa yɩ wɩ wɩɛ. Dɩ wɩ wer yaarʋra a sʋʋraa: Pɩɛr 'lar, ɩrɛ, a-n we fer.
41010050	Dɩ yaarʋ dʋna ɔɔ darã a faa, sa pal birbir da-n pɔ Jejura.
41010051	Dɩ Jeju bulee: Anye fɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋɛ far? Dɩ yaarʋ tu: Dɩɩrdaar, cʋɛ mɩ ma-n yɩ.
41010052	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dɩ kɔna, afɩ ha pɛ taa fɩ.
41010053	Dɩ dapaara ɔɔ yi khɛr da-n yɩ, a kpa Jejura dɩ wɩ cʋr wa-n jal.
41011001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n wɔrɔnɩ Jerujalɛm a ha Bɛtɩfaje na Betanɩ khʋra, wɩ kɔɔ daan gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔkɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra; le Jeju thɔ̃ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yenyɔ,
41011002	a so war ayɩ: Nɩ jala dɩɩraakɛ nɩ pɛnɩ ƴɩɛ; a nɩ pɔ na dã na yɩrɛ kũkə̃ ɓolʋʋkɛ tibil na jʋʋnnɩ pa', dɩ wa li; nɩ thʋba a kpa ɛna.
41011003	A tibil bule ni: Anye nɩ-n cʋʋ ya, nɩ to: Kɔ̃tɩn n ƴaalɛ sa a bir a thɔna kɔrɔ wɩ ɩna.
41011004	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ jal a yɩ kũkə̃ ɓolʋ, dɩ wɩ li cɔ lõfonɔɔ hʋ nʋɔra, dɩ wɩ thʋbɩ.
41011005	Dɩ ɩkhaa tibilsɔ wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ hanɩle bule wi: Anye nɩ-n cʋʋ, dɩ anyera nɩ-n thʋbɩ kũkə̃ ɓolʋ?
41011006	Dɩ kpãkpãadara gbaar mɔna Jeju kɔɔ so warnɩ a so war; dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ sɩ war dɩ wɩ jalna.
41011007	Dɩ wɩ pɔnanɛ kũkə̃ ɓolʋ Jejura, a gba awɩ kẽkẽ a dɛbɩ kũkəənə, dɩ Jeju jʋʋn tooro.
41011008	Tɩbɩla bərəəm kɔɔ belle awɩ kẽkẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ a pɛr hʋɛra, sɩ wɛ cɩ fa huu lɔɔ dɩ wa-n pɛr hʋɛra.
41011009	Wɩrɛ kʋlɛnɩ Jeju ƴɩɛ na wɩrɛ n kpaanɛnɩ khiro n hulene aa: Ojana, bɔnanɛ n hana ʋrɛraakɛ n ɩnanɩ gɩrɛ na Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i.
41011010	Bɔnanɛ n hana fãga gbaarraakɛ n ɩnanɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Davɩdɩɩda. Ojana le ƴũ pər.
41011011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju danɩ Jerujalɛm, a lʋʋn Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna; ɔbɔɔkɛ a hɩɩnnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ pɩ, a ther jal Betanɩ na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ gɩdonɩ dɩɩ kɔɔ 'lire tɩɩn.
41011012	A dɩɩ kɔɔ wɩl dɩ wɩ the Betanɩ, kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋrɛ Jeju.
41011013	Dɩ mɔ̃ a 'laanɩ yɩ thɩr khonanɛ ƴɔɔ dɩ thɔɔ faa, a gbaar pɔ ɩnɩ-n hɩɩn a ba sɛr yaa? Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ danɩ, fa haar dɩbara a kɔɔ yɩ, gɩdonɩ ga do ɔɔ se bɔ ga.
41011014	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju so thɩrʋraale ayɩ: Tibil na bir na kho afɩ bi kpɩɩrakɛ bã; dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ.
41011015	Agɩpɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan Jerujalɛm, dɩ Jeju lõ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, a ma a weele wɩrɛ n dolonenɩ thɩ̃ɛ na wɩrɛ n thɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, a tʋɔrna war debaa tabalsɔ a kpɛɛ na kʋlã puu dolõdaraa too pasɔ.
41011016	Sɩ aa-n tu tibil n fɔrɔ thɩ̃ɛ a kpãsɛnɛna Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna ga.
41011017	Sɩ a dɩɩr wɛr thakɛ aa: Ga do gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Mɛr Thãgbaa cɔ na dor paarɩkɛ tibil caar fɛʋ na-n fʋɔr mɩnaa”? Sɩ dɩ ne wer cʋʋ dɩɩ do yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaraa wɔ̃ pa.
41011018	Bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ gele dɩ wa-n ƴaal mɔ̃ wa fʋnɩ sɩ wɩ kʋ Jeju, gɩdonɩ a-n kʋ wɛr maar, gɩdonɩ nʋɔ n kpaarɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ ɔɔ dɩɩrra.
41011019	A dɩɩ birə Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara faarɛ dɩɩ sa the.
41011020	Dɩɩ wɩlnɩ duuro dɩ wa ka kpãkpãadara yɩrɛ thɩrʋʋlera dɩ khi na nɛɛ fɛʋ.
41011021	Dɩ Pɩɛr jɩna gɩrɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ a so Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, hɩnɛ thɩrʋʋkɛ fɩ pɛrnɩ sor a khire.
41011022	Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɩ pɩɛr Thãgba haar.
41011023	Sobɔr mɩ so nar: A tibil so gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔkɛ ayɩ: Ǝlə kɩɛr a je lanyʋɔnna, dɩ ado ntɛ na baalɔ ɔɔ hara ga, sa pɛr haar gɩrɛ ɩnɩ sonɩ ga har oti, a na yɩɛrɛ ga cʋʋna gel.
41011024	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so nar: Thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na bɩɛlnɩ Thãgbara, nɩ pɩɛr haar nɩ 'lɛr pɩ, dɩ na yɩɛrɛ gɩ cʋʋna.
41011025	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ ɩɩrnɩ jɩɩl na bɩɛl Thãgba, ado nɩ hananɛ sor na tibil, nɩ faa, dɩ mɛ̃ anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ na faa dakha anɩ sopugo.
41011026	[Sɩ ado na faa wɩ̃ tibili soa', anɩ Thɩɩkɛ hanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ na faa dakha anɩ sopugoə'.l
41011027	Dɩ wɩ bire jal Jerujalɛm, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n kpaarnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na kɔ̃tɩna pʋɔraarɛ,
41011028	a bulee: Ka hʋ caakɛra fɩ hananɩ dɩ fa-n cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛɛkɛra the, dɩ amɛ hana fɩ hʋɛ fa-n cʋɛ?
41011029	Dɩ Jeju tu: Ma bule ner dakha thɩ̃ bɩɛl, a nɩ puno birse mi mɛrɛ dakha ma so narɛ hʋ ca ʋrɛ mɩ hananɩ dɩ ma-n cʋʋna thɩ̃ ca gɩrɛ.
41011030	Jãa yɔ kpɛɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ the yaa, tɩbɩlaa pa gɩ the? Nɩ to ɩ̃ hɩɩn.
41011031	Dɩ wɩ mar dɩ wa-n bana khasɔ ayɩ: A sɩ tu ayɩ: Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ the, a na bule ser dɩ anye dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ sa kɔɔ pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haara';
41011032	dɩ a sɩ so wo ayɩ: Tɩbɩlaa pa gɩ... Maar kɔɔ fʋɔn wɩ tɩbɩlala thalee sora, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa bobon bɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ kɔɔ gba Jã dɩ do.
41011033	Dɩ wɩ tu: Sɩ jɩrɛ ya? Dɩ Jeju so war: Dɩ a thale gɩ, ma-n so nar mer ka mɩ yɩnɩ hʋɛ dɩ ma-n cʋʋna ga thɩ̃sɔɔka'.
41012001	Jeju mar da-n mɩɩ wɩ na sokpaa ayɩ: Kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ cʋʋ nãkʋɔr a bã dãgbol diiro, a kpena dakha koru bi der paar, sa mɩ bɛbɛr cɔ gbãa. Agɩpɩ dɩ gba nãkʋɔr hɩɩndara a pɛr wa-n hɩnɛ ɓo, sa jal kpaar paar.
41012002	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ bi khʋ̃ bɔɔ danɩ, a thʋɔn ɔɔ thɔ̃daar bɩɛl a jala nãkʋɔr hɩɩndararara, wɩ hanaa dɩkhaa nãkʋɔr thɩ̃ a pɔna.
41012003	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ thɔ̃daar a bɩɩr, sa weguu dɩ kɔna nyɛ̃ khɩɩ.
41012004	Dɩ bir thɔ̃ war thɔ̃daar kpɩɩ wo, dɩ wɩ bɩɩrʋʋ yʋʋ cu, sa pɩɛraa yicuru.
41012005	Dɩ bir thɔ̃ war thɔ̃daar kpɩɩ wo, dɩ wɩ kʋʋ. Agɩpɩ dɩ thɔ̃ war wɩ̃ thɔ̃dara wo, dɩ wɩ fʋlɛlɛ wɛ a bɩɩr sa kʋʋr ɩkha.
41012006	Sɩɩ do ɔɔ bikũu bɩɛlɩkɛ a-n nanɩ sɩɛraa, dɩ pɩɩrɔ thʋ̃ɔ wɛrra sa so wa cʋrɛ ɩ̃ bikuun.
41012007	Sɩ nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaraale mɩɩrɛ kha ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn thɩ̃ hɩn, nɩ dɔ sɩ kʋʋ, sɩɩ do sɛr hɩna thɩ̃ɛ.
41012008	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ fʋʋ, a kʋʋ, a gba dʋna faa nãkʋɔr khuirə.
41012009	Anye nãkʋɔr kɔ̃tɩn na cʋʋ dɩphã? A na jaal na kʋʋr nãkʋɔr hɩɩndaraale, sa a gba nãkʋɔr a ha tɩɩ kpɩɩsɔ.
41012010	A thɩɛna gaa, na kɔɔ hɩɩn gɩrɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonaa? Gɩ sor ayɩ: “Bokaarɩkɛ cɔ mɛ kɔɔ bonɩ, debire a do go tɩ bokaar;
41012011	sɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ pa thɩ̃ɛɛle the, dɩ sɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ do sar thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ.”
41012012	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ hʋɛ wɩ fʋʋ, sɩɩ do maar n fʋ wɛr tɩbɩlala, gɩdonɩ wɩ jɩrɛ dɩ wɛrra Jeju so sokpaale, sɩ wɩ kɔɔ fagʋʋrɛ sa kɔ̃.
41012013	Sɩ wɩ thʋɔnaanɛ ɩkhaa jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ totoo, wɩ nʋɔ thɩmɩɩrraakɛ a na mɩɩnɩ.
41012014	Dɩ wɩ pɔr a sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sobɔ tibil fɩ do, dɩ fa-n ma tibilə', fa-n hɩɩn dakha tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa', sɩ dɩ fa-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla Thãgbaa hʋ na sobɔr. Gɩ teere kha dɩ sa lɩmɩ Sejaar lãpho yaa, ga tee kha ga?
41012015	Sɩ lɩma yaa, sa-n lɩma? Sɩ gɩdonɩ Jeju jɩrɛ awɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔ fɩl, a so warɛ: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n fifilə mi? Nɩ gba war bi bɩɛl ɛna ɩ̃ hɩɩn.
41012016	Dɩ wɩ gba bɩɛl a pɔna, dɩ bule wi: Amɛɛ foto ha ʋrɛ, dɩ amɛɛ khere ha gɩrɛ? Dɩ wɩ tu: Sejaar gɩ.
41012017	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju so war: Nɩ 'laanɛ Sejaarra gɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ Sejaarɩda, a 'laanɛ Thãgbara gɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaada; dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɛr fɛʋ ɔrra.
41012018	Dɩ Sadʋsɛ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala', pʋɔraarɛ a bulee thakɛ ayɩ:
41012019	Dɩɩrdaar, hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ khere sarnɩ ayɩ: “Ado tibil hana õkuun dɩ khi sa faa khɛr sɩ bɩsaan na hala', ɔɔ õkuun n gba hɛ a kɔna bɩsana wɩ do ɔɔ õkuuni məl.”
41012020	Sɩɩ do õkona makonyɔ wɛ a kɔɔ hale; cacadaar kɔɔ her khɛr aa hana bɩsana ga, sa khi.
41012021	Dɩ balanyɔdaar gba khikhɛrʋ aa hana bɩsana ga, sa khi wo; mɛna gɩ kɔɔ ha dakha na balãtherdaar.
41012022	Sɩ bɩɛl wɛr makonyɔrarakɛ na hana bɩsaana', wɩ pɩnɩ fɛʋ na pɩ dɩɩ do khɛr dakha khire.
41012023	Ado khe ɩɩr khirera, ʋmɔ̃ wɛrra na hɩna khɛr? Gɩdonɩ wɛr makonyɔra fɛʋʋ khɛr a kɔɔ do.
41012024	Dɩ Jeju tu: Nɩ buure waa fu yə̃ə? Na jɩnɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ na Thãgbaa fãga ga, gɛr gɩ.
41012025	Ado khe na ɩɩr khirera, kona na he khɛra bã, khɛra dakha na he kona bã, sɩ wa hʋrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ le Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
41012026	Sɩ ado gɩrɛ dɔnɩ khee ɩɩr gɩ, na kɔɔ yɩɛ Mʋɩjɩɩ sɛbɛra thɩr bu thɩmɩɩrra gaa? Mee Thãgbaa sʋʋraarɛ ayɩ: “Ɩnɛr dʋɔn Abɩrahamɩ Thãgba, na Ɩjakɩɩ Thãgba, na Jakɔbɩɩ Thãgba.”
41012027	Thãgba na do khee Thãgba ga, sɩ wɩrɛ hananɩ yiree Thãgba a do; nɩ bure waa vʋ̃ʋ.
41012028	Jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar bɩɛlɩkɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n bananɩ thɩ̃ banaa, a jɩna dakha mɔ̃ Jeju jɩɩnɩ tu, a pɔr a bulee ayɩ: Ʋmɔ̃ dɔ caca jɔfʋ jɔfʋsɔra fɛʋ?
41012029	Dɩ Jeju tu: Gacadaa dʋɔn: “Ɩjɩrayɛl na pɛ nũu, Kɔ̃tɩn asɩ Thãgba, Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ a do,
41012030	dɩ dɔ fa-n na Kɔ̃tɩn afɩ Thãgba na afɩ bɩ̃ fɛʋ, na afɩ ha fɛʋ, na afɩ kpɩɛr fɛʋ, na afɩ fãga fɛʋ.”
41012031	Balanyɔdaa dʋɔn: “Dɔ fa-n na afɩ 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃kɛ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara.” Jɔfʋ na hale a kɔ̃tɩ̃ jɔ jɔfʋ ca ƴɩrɛ bã.
41012032	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar sʋʋraa: Gɩ bɔrɛ Dɩɩrdaar, sobɔr fɩ so, dɩ bɩɛl Thãgba do 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ, dakpɩɩ na hale saagado ɔr gaaga,
41012033	dɩ ɔɔ naakɛ fa-n naanɩ na bɩnɛ fɛʋ, na kpɩɛrɛ fɛʋ, na fãga fɛʋ, fa-n nana dakha 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara, gɩ jɔr nʋmaakɛ wɩ-n jinəni bonɩɛ Thãgbara sa thii, na gɩ̃ bonɩ ji fɛʋ.
41012034	A Jeju yɩ mɔ̃ a tuni thale na kpɛsɛrɛ, a sʋʋraarɛ: Fa hʋnɔ dɩ Thãgba na do far fãgadaara'. Dɩ tibil na 'la na bule Jeju thɩ̃ɛ bã.
41012035	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju hanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna da-n dɩɩr wɩ, a sor ayɩ: Mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na-n so ayɩ: Davɩdɩɩ Bikuun Kirisiti do?
41012036	Davɩdɩɩ thɛthɛ Thu Phuu kɔɔ cʋʋ dɩ so ayɩ: “Thãgba sor ɩ̃ Kɔ̃tɩna ayɩ: Tɔɔ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra, phaphapha ɩ̃ cʋʋ afɩ lãlaardara wɩ do afɩ nɛ jəəda.”
41012037	Davɩdɩɩ thɛthɛrakɛ n wɩɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ mɔ̃ a na fʋ sɩ na do ɔɔ bikuun? Tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ pɛr Jeju nũu na daʋ.
41012038	Dɩ a-n dɩɩrɛ tɩbɩla ayɩ: Na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔɔkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩnɩ-n tɔ kẽkẽ gbana na kpaarna ƴatɔɔ tɩbɩla na-n fʋɔrɛ nɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋ;
41012039	ɩnɩ-n phiirna ƴɛ kʋʋl too paar Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ, na caca too paar dɩko kho paar;
41012040	ɩna-n phʋʋna khikhɛra, sɩɩ do fɩɩlɛ wɩ-n bɩɛlna Thãgba dɩ wa-n pʋɔrna wa-n yɛ nɩ; wele, so kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na heen wer na khɩɩr na ka.
41012041	Jeju toore a pɛ ka wɩ-n pɛnɩ Thãgba mũsumo ƴɩɛ, da-n hɩɩn mɔ̃ tibil jɔɔle n pɛrnɩ war Thãgba mũsũ pɛ paar. Lẽledara bərəəm pɛrɛ war jɔɔ.
41012042	Dɩ khikhɛr bɔdaar pɔ a pɛr tama be yenyɔɔkɛ na dananɩ war birə'.
41012043	Dɩ Jeju we ɔɔ kpãkpãadara a so war: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, khikhɛrʋʋkɛ pɛrɛ war dɩɩ jɔ gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋ pɛrnɩ Thãgba mũsũ pɛ paar.
41012044	Gɩdonɩ war harra wɩrɛ fɛʋ pɛr, sɩ ɔr, ɔɔ bɔdaar warɩkɛ a hananɩ koo, kɛ na haanɛɛnɩ a pɛr.
41013001	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju n thenɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, ɔɔ kpãkpãadaar bɩɛl sʋʋraarɛ: Dɩɩrdaar, yɛ boka ɓɔnanakɛ, dɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ wɩ thʋnɩ mɩ gʋʋsɔ ɓoɓo.
41013002	Dɩ Jeju birsee ayɩ: Fa yɩ mɔ̃ wɩ thʋnɩ mɩ go kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔkɛ ɓoɓoaa? Boka bɩɛl na bir na sɩ kɩɛr na dɛ̃ɛ ʋ̃ bokara ƴũ bã, fɛʋ na derre.
41013003	Mɔ̃ Jeju toonɩ gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra a pɛ ƴɩɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, Pɩɛr na Jakɩ na Jã na Ãdire kɔɔ buleele hɛllɩ:
41013004	Sɔ sar bɔɔkɛ gelela na danɩ, dɩ anye dɔ jɩɩnɩkɛ na nɛnanɩ bɔɔkɛ gelesɔra na-n danɩ.
41013005	Dɩ Jeju ma da-n so war ayɩ: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, na-n do tibil n fɩɩl na'.
41013006	Gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla bərəəm na gbaar ɩ̃ i na ɩna wa-n so, ɩnɛr dʋɔn mɛrɛ; dɩ mɛ̃ wa fɩɩl tɩbɩla jɔɔ.
41013007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ nɩɛnɩ kʋʋr hale na mɔ̃ na-n nɩɛnɩ ko thɩmɩasɔ, na-n do maar n fʋ na', dɔ gele n kɔɔ dã sɩ ga do thɩ pɩ paar pa'.
41013008	Ʋ ca na ɩɩrɛ a na-n kena ʋ̃ ca, ʋ̃ fãgadaarɩ dɩ bɩɛl n ɩɩr a na-n kena ʋ̃ fãgadaarɩ dɩ kpɩɩ. Thɩ jɩɩnsɔ na har paar dɩɩdɩɩ, kɔmɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na jire dakha; sɩ gɩrɛ wallɛɛ tɔ̃tʋ̃ɔ pa gɩ.
41013009	Sɩ na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ dɩbara, gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla na fʋ nɛr na jalna kɩɩl paar; wa bɩɩr nɛr dakha Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ; wa kpa nɛr na jalna dɩ na jɩɩl gobanɛrsɔ na fãgadarasɔɔ ƴɛra, gɩ do mɛr dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ ga mɩɩ warɛ anɩ ha pɛda.
41013010	Dɔ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ n kɔɔ mɩɩ tibil caarra fɛʋ ɓo.
41013011	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ fʋ nɩnɩ a jalna kɩɩl paar, na-n kɔɔ ma na dɛ anye na so yaa ga, sɩ dawiilera thɩmɩɩr na the ner nɔɔ dɩ na so, gɩdonɩ ga do anɩ pa ga tha', sɩ Thu Phʋʋ na hana nɩ.
41013012	Õkuun na liirnanɛ ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔ dɩ wa kʋ, ɔmɛ̃ thɩrɛ na cʋʋ na ɔɔ bɩsã; bɩsana na ɩɩrɛ na lã thɩrɛ na nɩrɛra.
41013013	Tɩbɩla fɛʋ na laar nɛr gɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na yɩranɩ a na dana khu paar, ɔr na 'lɛ taarɛ.
41013014	Ɔbɔɔkɛ na yɩnɩ thɩ̃ thuurnəneekɛ na kʋɛanɩ thɩ̃ɛ da ha kãkɛ na teananɩ a hana ga (dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ n hɩnɛnɩ sɛbɛɛkɛ n dʋ gar bʋrɛ), le wɩrɛ hanɩ Jude n fuo ca jala gɔ̃gʋɔna;
41013015	ʋrɛɛkɛ na hanɩ nãsʋrɔ a na-n gbũ lõ cʋɔrɔ ɩnɩ-n gba thɩ̃a';
41013016	dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ dakha na hanɩ lɔɔ a na-n kɛr bir ɩnɩ-n gba ɩnɩ kẽkẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bã.
41013017	Ga wisɔɔle ga puurore khɛ pɛmɛdarara na wɩrɛ n mamanɩ bibɔrɔsɔ.
41013018	Na-n bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba dɩ thɩ̃ɛ thale na-n dã yʋʋrɔa'.
41013019	Ga wisɔɔle bɔ gaarɛ na jɔrɛ na ka, bɔ gaar caale na kɔɔ hale ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ tini thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ dana nɛnɛ̃ka', dɩ ga bir na halerakɛ kpɩɩ bã.
41013020	Ado Kɔ̃tɩn na kɔɔ tɔ ga bɔɔle dɩɩ gburoə', tibil na mar na ta ga, sɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ a kɔɔ phiirni wɩ dɔ ɩnɩ too dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ tɔ ga bɔɔle dɩɩ gburo.
41013021	Liir ado tibil na so nar: Nɩ hɩnɛ Kirisiti har kɩɛr, agɩbo: Nɩ hɩnɛ pal a ha, na-n pɛr haara'.
41013022	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n sõsonenɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ Kirisiti ha nɩ, agɩbo bobona ha nɩ, na ɩɩrɛ wa-n nɩna tɩbɩla nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔ, wa-n fɩɩlnanakɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ phiirni adora wa punone.
41013023	Sɩ nɛrɛ, na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ koe; mɩ kɔɔ maanɛ dɩ ma-n so nar gɩrɛ fɛʋ.
41013024	Ga bɔɔlera a bɔ gaarɛ ka na pɩ, wire na birəre, por dakha na hɩrɛ bã.
41013025	Yepələ̃be na ther thãgbara ƴũ ga-n jiir thɩɩra, dɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ fãgaakɛ hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ ga gbugbuyore.
41013026	Le wa yɩ tibili Bikuun a na-n ɩ̃ na ndɔlɔ̃pana na fãga jɔɔ ka na carbararɛ jɔɔ.
41013027	Le a na thɔ̃ ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ dɩ wa kpa wɩrɛ a phiirni, kɛ hanɩ kɩrrɔ, na gananɔ, na gɛla yenyɔra, na ka thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩ khuni.
41013028	Nɩ dɔ sokpaa thɩr khonanɛdara n dɩɩrnɩ thɩ̃ɛ; ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ yɩnɩ ɔɔ jɛ̃ dɩɩ ɓol a na thɔɔ fa ƴolo, nɩ jɩrɛ ubulo n wɩla.
41013029	Mɛ̃ gɩ, nɛrɛ dakha a nɩ yɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ dɩ a dã, nɩ jɛ tibili Bikuuni ɩ̃ bɔ n daan, dɩ lõfonɔɔ a ha.
41013030	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, nĩdaraakɛ na khiir koo sɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ fɛʋ n dã ga.
41013031	Thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩ na phor na ka, sɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔ na pho na ka kpɩɩraka'.
41013032	Ado wi jɩɩrra gɩ, na bɔɔkɛ ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ na danɩ, tibil bɩɛl na ja', thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔrakɛ le Thãgbaa dʋɔ wa ja', mɛr Bikuunnakɛ na ja', sɩ Thɩrɛ dɩbara jɩɛn.
41013033	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ a na jʋrɛna, gɩdonɩ na jɩ bɔɔkɛ ga dana'.
41013034	Ga hʋrɛ mɔ̃ tibil n pɛrnɩ haar ɩna jaal dɩkhãa pa, dɩ faa cʋɔr sɩ dɩ 'laa ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔra bɩɛlbɩɛl hʋɛ thɔmanaakɛ wa-n donɩ, sɩ dɩ so lo bɛrdaarra, a na-n jɩɛ jʋʋr.
41013035	Na-n jʋrɛ mɛ̃, gɩdonɩ na jɩ bɔɔkɛ cɔdaar kuun na birni na ɩ̃a'; agakpaana dʋɔrɔ ga do, agɩbo dɩnɩrɔ, a mɛ̃ gaa yɔl ko khɩɩ bɔɔ, agɩbo duuro.
41013036	Ado a phuro a ɩ̃ na-n do a fʋ nɩ daanɔa'.
41013037	Gɩrɛ mɩ so narnɩ, tɩbɩlala fɛʋ mɩ so: A nɩ jɩ na-n jʋrɛ.
41014001	Wire yenyɔ sɛra sɩɩ do Pakɩ ɓol bɔɔ na buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraa kho bɔ daan. Le bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara n ƴaal hʋɛ wɩ fʋ Jeju na fɩɩlɛ wɩ kʋ.
41014002	Gɩdonɩ wɩ n sor, ɩna fʋʋ ɓol bɔa', a mɛ̃ gaa khʋ̃ɛ na ɩɩrɛ tibil jɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
41014003	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju hanɩ Betanɩ Sɩmɔ̃ gbuuluu cɔ dɩko kho paar, khɛ bɩɛl lʋʋn le, a fʋrɔ laaso ja bulabirikɛ hananɩ latɩkolookɛ n hʋnanɩ daʋ, a khɩɩr the nʋɔ ka; dɩ a cʋɔrɛ bulobirile a deer latɩkolo Jejuu yʋɔ.
41014004	Dɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ hanɩle nĩkhii fʋ wɛr dɩ wa-n so: Anyee latɩkolo kʋɛ ca ha gɩrɛ thakɛ?
41014005	Ga do wa kɔɔ dolonena gɩ dã wire tãatherɩɩ thɔ̃ lɩmɩ wɩ ha bɔdara gaa? Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ cɩ̃cɩma khɛrraale.
41014006	Sɩ Jeju so: Nɩ sɩɛraa, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n vɔgʋʋ? Thɔ̃ bʋɔ a cʋʋ mar;
41014007	gɩdonɩ bɔdara n har wire fɛʋ anɩ pa, nɩ punone cʋʋ wɩ bɔɔ mɔ̃ nɩ-n ƴaalnɩ, sɩ mɛrɛ na hana mɩ khorra'.
41014008	Gɩrɛ a-n punoni ha gɩrɛ a cʋʋnɩ, a kɔɔ mãa a thir mi latɩkolo da-n gbɛbɩ mɩ mɔ̃ wa dʋ mɩnɩ.
41014009	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, paar fɛʋʋkɛ wa mɩɩnɩ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ thɩɩraakɛ fɛʋ, wa mɩɩrɛ dakha gɩrɛɛkɛ khɛrɩkɛ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ dɩ wa jɩnaa.
41014010	Sɩ Judasɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ dɩɩra, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ kpãkpãadaar bɩɛl yʋɔr yenyɔra, jaal bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnaa pa dɩ a na liirna Jeju.
41014011	Dɩɩ da war na sobɔr mɔ̃ a-n mɩɩ wɩnɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ, ɩɩɩa haarɛ war. Dɩ Judasɩ jɩɩ ma da-n ƴaal hʋɛ waa a liirnaa.
41014012	Buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraa caca ɓol wi, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ wireekɛ wɩ-n jinəni Pakɩ bana bire bonɩɛ, Jejuu kpãkpãadara buleele ayɩ: Ka fɩ-n ƴaal sɩ jala gbɛbɩrɛ Pakɩ dɩkor fɩ kho?
41014013	Dɩ a thʋɔn ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yenyɔ a so war ayɩ: Nɩ jala dɩɩra, kuunikɛ heenenɩ nyʋɔn na daa na caana nɛr, na-n kpaaraa,
41014014	dɩ ka a na lonɩ nɩ sɔ cɔdaar kuunna ayɛ: Dɩɩrdaar yɩ, ka duukɛ ɩna khoronɩ Pakɩ dɩkor na ɩnɩ kpãkpãadara ha?
41014015	Dɩ a na nɩ narɛ lɩ̃gã kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ wɩ thɩɩnɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ, nɩ gbɛbɩrɛ le Pakɩ dɩkor.
41014016	Dɩ kpãkpãadara jaal a dã dɩɩra, a yɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ ha mɔna Jeju kɔɔ so warnɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ gbɛbɩ Pakɩ dɩkor.
41014017	A dɩɩ dʋɔr Jeju pɔr na yʋɔr yenyɔ.
41014018	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ toonɩ dɩ wa-n kho dɩkor Jeju sor: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛraakɛ sɩ-n khonanɩ kha dɩkor na liirna mɛr.
41014019	Dɩ wɩ ma dɩ wa-n gbobi, sɩ dɩ wɛr bɩɛlbɩɛl na-n bulee ɩnɛr gɩ kã?
41014020	Dɩ birse wi: Tibil bɩɛl nɛr yʋɔr yenyɔraakɛ n 'lɔɔnɩ tasa bɩɛl na mɛrɛ gɩ.
41014021	Mɛr tibili Bikuun n jaal mɔ̃kɛ gɩ khere marnɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra, sɩ ga puure ʋrɛraakɛ na lirenanɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun; a wa kɔɔ kɔ̃ tibil ca olelaka', gɩ ka baar.
41014022	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n khonɩ dɩkor Jeju gbaar buru, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a kuure a ha wɩ sa so: Nɩ gba gɩrɛra ɩ̃ tomɩ gɩ.
41014023	Agɩpɩ dɩ gba thɩ̃ yɔnanɛ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a fʋɔrnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a ha wɛr, dɩ wɛr fɛʋ gba a yɔ.
41014024	Dɩ a so warɛ aa: Gɩrɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃, Thãgbaa nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ tɔmɩ̃ gɩ, a na deer tɩbɩla bərəəm sora.
41014025	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ma bir na yɔ dɩvɛ̃ɛkɛ bã, phaphapha gɩ dana wireekɛ ma birni na yɔ daphaa Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dʋɔ.
41014026	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ khɩnɩ nɩɛ pɩ, wɩ ther jal gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra.
41014027	Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɛrɛ fɛʋ na kɛrnanɛ khiru, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Mɛr Thãgba na bɩɩrɛ bana khedaar dɩ banaa na bɩ̃bɩlã paar fɛʋ.”
41014028	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ma ɩɩrnɩ na the khirera ma kʋʋl nɛr ƴɩɛ na jal Galile.
41014029	Dɩ Pɩɛr sʋʋraa: Ado tɩbɩla fɛʋrakɛ na kɛrnanɛ khiru, sɩ me wer ma kɛrna khiruə'.
41014030	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Sobɔr mɩ so far, fɛrɛ, nĩ dɩtɩnɔɔkɛ yɔl kʋʋ na khɩɩrakɛ balanyɔa', sɩ balãther fa bana nayɩ fa jɩ ma'.
41014031	Sɩ Pɩɛr bir tu na kheu: Adorakɛ wɩ yɩ sɩ khe kha, sɩ ma puno na bana nayɩ ma jɩ faa ga; dɩ mɛ̃ wɛr fɛʋ kɔɔ so dakha.
41014032	Agɩpɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jɛcɛmanɛ, dɩ Jeju so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Nɩ tɔɔ kɩɛr ɔbɔɔkɛ ma hanɩ Thãgba bɩɛllɔ.
41014033	Dɩ a kpar Pɩɛr na Jakɩ na Jã, sɩ maar mar dɩ ga-n fʋʋ, dɩ haar haa kũkulõo.
41014034	Dɩ a so warɛ: Ɩ̃ ha gbobire khikhi gbobire waa gel, nɩ tɔɔ kɩɛr a na jʋrɛ.
41014035	Mɛ̃ a tɔ jal gbe, a ji thɩɩra da-n bɩɛl Thãgba adora hʋɛ hale gɩ dora bɔ̃ gaar bɔɔle khokhɩaraarɛ,
41014036	a sor aa: Aba (kɩrʋ dʋɔn Thɩrɛ), fɛr n punone thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, hʋnɔnɛ mar thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ sɩ ga do mɔ̃ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ ga, sɩ mɔ̃ fɛrɛ n pɛrnɩ haar gɩ hana.
41014037	Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ kɛr pɔ war a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa-n daar, dɩ so Pɩɛrra: Sɩmɔ̃, fɛr n daarɛɛ? Fa kɔɔ puno toorakɛ gbe a jʋʋr hɩɩnaa?
41014038	Nɩ jʋrɛ a na bɩɛlna Thãgba dɩ mɛ̃ na lõ fifiləlela ga. Tuur wer n har haarra gel, sɩ tibili tibil do pa fãga 'lee.
41014039	Dɩ mɛ̃ a kɛr jal wo da-n bɩɛl Thãgba da-n 'loro mɔ̃kɛra a kɔɔ sonɩ.
41014040	Sɩ a bire pɔ wo, a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa-n daar, gɩdonɩ dayuur fʋ wɛr a kar, dɩ wa jɩ mɔ̃ wa sʋʋraana'.
41014041	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a pɔ warnɩ dɩɩ dã balãther, a so warɛ: Nɩ daarɛ dɩphã a hɩrɛ; gɩ daan dɩ bɔɔ daan. Nɩ hɩnɛ, wa liirnanɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun sopugodara.
41014042	Nɩ ɩrɛ sɩ jal, sɩ hɩnɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ lirena mɩnɩ n ɩnɛ.
41014043	Mɔ̃ a hanɩ mɩɩrɔ, dapaara Judasɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ bɩɛl kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔra daan na tibil jɔɔkɛ fɔrɔnɩ bajɩnasɔ na gbolasɔ, kɛ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ kɔɔ thɔnɩ.
41014044	Sɩ lĩlir kɔɔ nɩ warɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ a na cʋʋnɩ aa, ʋrɛɛkɛ ɩna palnɩ, ɔr gɩ, wɩ fʋɔnɛɛ jalana sɩ wa-n do a yɩ fuu paara'.
41014045	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a danɩ, dapaara a tɔ wɔrɔ̃ Jeju sa so: Dɩɩrdaar; sa palʋʋ.
41014046	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ Jeju.
41014047	Sɩ tibil bɩɛl wɛrra pher bajɩna, a cɩna Thãgbaa gbõdaarɩ thɔ̃daar nũu a kur.
41014048	Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɩ ɩanɛ bajɩna na gbolasɔ nɩ fʋ mɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n fʋnɩ yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaar koe.
41014049	Mɩ-n kɔɔ har kha na nɛrɛ wire fɛʋ dɩ ma-n dɩɩr nɩ thɩ̃ɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, sɩ na kɔɔ fʋ ma'. Sɩ gɩ har thakɛ gɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ gɩ dã.
41014050	Liir wɩ fuule fɛʋ sa fagʋʋ.
41014051	Sɩ daɓol bɩɛl gɩ da-n kɔɔ kpa Jejura, a par kẽkẽ nɩɩ, wɩ fʋʋrɛ,
41014052	dɩ for kelẽ nɩɩ pɛ war sa cana sãɓɔlɔ̃.
41014053	Dɩ wɩ kpar Jeju a jalna gbõdaarɩ pa ka bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ n gbɛbɩnɩ kha.
41014054	Sɩ Pɩɛr n kpaar Jejura nɔ bɩɛl nɔ bɩɛl, a ba dana gbõdaarɩ gbaya, a lõ too le na thɔ̃dara da-n ɩɩr dɔɔ.
41014055	Bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na so gʋʋrdara fɛʋ, kɔɔ kpɛr sɔ dɩ wa-n pɛ Jeju wɩ yɩrɔ hʋɛ wɩ kʋʋ, sɩ wa kɔɔ yɩ ga.
41014056	Sɩ tibil jɔ kɔɔ pɔr a kuur sɔ̃sɔ dɩ wa-n pɛ Jejura, sɩ awɩ so jɩ na ma kha ga.
41014057	Dɩ ɩkhasɔ n ɩɩr dɩ wɩ sõso na pɩɛraa ayɩ,
41014058	ɩnɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ so ayɩ, ɩna kʋɛrɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ tɩbɩla mɩnɩ, sɩ ɩnɩ-n bir ɩnɩ-n mɩ dakpɩɩ wire balãther, sɩ ga do tibil nyɛ̃ɛ ma'.
41014059	Sɩ gelelakɛ wɩ sonɩ awɩ so jɩ na ma kha ga.
41014060	Dɩ gbõdaar pal ɩɩr tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn a bule Jeju: Fa-n hana nʋɔ na birsena gaa? Anyee so ha gɩrɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ n pɛ farnɩ?
41014061	Sɩ Jeju pɩr pɔbɩ aa əl nʋɔa', dɩ gbõdaar bir bulee: Sɩɩ do fɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti, Thãgbaakɛ sɩ-n fʋɔrnɩɩ Bikuun bɛ?
41014062	Dɩ Jeju tu: Mɛrra gɩ, sɩ na yɩrɛ tibili Bikuun da too Thãgbaa nyɔ̃bɔra, a thena dakha thãgbara ƴũ a na-n ɩ̃ na ndɔlɔ̃pana.
41014063	Dɩ gbõdaar ɓəər ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ sa so: Anye hale dɩ sa bir na 'lo dɩkha 'lo?
41014064	Nɩ nɩɛnɩ mɔ̃ a kʋɛnɩ Thãgbaa i; mɔ̃ nɩ-n kpɩɛr? Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ pɩɛraa so kʋnanɛ.
41014065	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ wɛrra mar dɩ wa-n cɩɩraa nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ, sa thii ƴɩɛ sɩ dɩ wa-n thʋʋrʋʋ na nyɔ̃ po, sɩ wa-n sʋʋraa a jɛ ntɛ n bɩɛnɩ; sɩ thɔ̃dara gbaarɛ sɩ wa-n ɓaalɛ.
41014066	Mɔ̃ Pɩɛr hanɩ gbayara, gbõdaar thɔ̃daar khɛ bɩɛl pɔr
41014067	a yɩɩ da-n ɩɩr dɔɔ, dɩ hɩɩnʋʋ kirkirkɩr sa sʋʋraa. Fɛrɛ dakha mee fɩ-n kɔɔ ha kha na Najarɛtɩ Jeju.
41014068	Sɩ a bananɛ sa so: Ma ja', ma-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ fɩ ƴaalnɩ fɩ soa'. Agɩpɩ Pɩɛr gba jal thena phel ko lõfonʋɔ.
41014069	Dɩ thɔ̃daar khɛrɩle yɩɩ, a bir ma da-n so wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩle aa: Kuunikɛ wa tibil cara bɩɛl gɩ.
41014070	Sɩ Pɩɛr bir da-n bana wo. Bɔɔ gbe dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hanɩle bir sʋʋraa: Sobɔr gɩ gel, wa tibil ca bɩɛl fɩ do gɩdonɩ Galiledaar ha fɩ.
41014071	Sɩ Pɩɛr mar a bana a ʋlfɛ da-n wɩɩrna thɩ̃ɛsɔ aa, ɩna jɩ kuunikɛ wɩ-n sona'.
41014072	Dɩ dapaara balanyɔ yɔl kʋʋ bir khɩɩ, dɩ Pɩɛr jɩna Jejuu thɩmɩɩkɛ a kɔɔ sʋʋraanɩ ayɩ, a yɔl kʋʋ na 'lɛ na khɩɩ balanyɔa', sɩ a na bananɛ balãther nayɩ, ɩna jɩ na'. Dɩ mɔ̃ Pɩɛr n kpɩɛrnɩ thale a-n khɩɩrɛ.
41015001	A dɩɩ wɩl duuro phiphi, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ, na so gʋʋrdara fɛʋ gbɛbɩrɛ kha wɩ gʋʋr mɔ̃ wa donɩ. A wɩ li Jeju pɩ, wɩ kpaarɛ ha Pɩlatɩ.
41015002	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ bulee ayɩ: Fɛr dʋɔn Juifi fãgadaarɩ? Dɩ Jeju tu: Mɔna fɩ sonɩ gɩ.
41015003	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna pɩɛraa sɔ jɔɔjɔɔ.
41015004	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ bir bulee wo: Fa-n hana nʋɔ na birsena gaa? Hɩnɛ sɔ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ-n pɛ farnɩ.
41015005	Sɩ Jeju na kɔɔ so thɩ̃ɛ bã, dɩ gɛr cʋɛ dɩ nʋɔ kpaa Pɩlatɩ.
41015006	Sɩ ɓol bɔɔ fɛʋ Pɩlatɩ n faarɛ khaɩdaarɩkɛ tɩbɩla n ƴaalnɩ.
41015007	Sɩ tibil bɩɛl hale khaɩra wɩ-n wenɩ Barabasɩ nakha lãlana, gɩdonɩ tibil wɩ kɔɔ kʋ dawiikɛ wɩ kɔɔ ɩɩrnanɩ lãʋ.
41015008	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle jʋʋnɛ Pɩlatɩɩ pa, a ma dɩ wa-n bɩɛlʋʋ a cʋɛ nar gɩrɛɛkɛ a-n kɔɔ cʋʋ narnɩ.
41015009	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ tu: Nɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ faa ʋrɛ dɔnɩ Juifi fãgadaar a ha nɩ ya?
41015010	Gɩdonɩ a jɩrɛ dɩ gbugi dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna kɔɔ fʋ Jeju a haa.
41015011	Sɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna cʋrrɛ tɩbɩla wa-n pɛr, wɩ sɔ Pɩlatɩra a ka faa Barabasɩ.
41015012	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ bir bule wi: Sɩ anye nɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋɛna ʋrɛ nɩ-n wenɩ Juifr fãgadaar?
41015013	Dɩ wɩ tu kheu wɛlɛ wɛlɛ aa: Gbaanɛɛ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
41015014	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ bule wi: Anyee puu ca a cʋʋ? Sɩ wɩ bir tu na kheu wɛlɛ wɛlɛ dɩɩ jɔ mɛ̃ aa: Gbaanɛɛ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
41015015	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n da tibil jɔ haar a faa Barabasɩ, sa gba Jeju 'laa dɩ wɩ ciil na khasa sɩ dɩ ha wɩ wɩ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
41015016	Dɩ sɔrasɛ kɔɔ kpar Jeju a lona gobanɛrɩ cɔ gbayara, dɩ wɩ wer wɩ̃ sɔrasɩsɔ fɛʋ.
41015017	Sɩ wɩ tor Jeju kẽkẽ sɩɛ, a kɛrna uu dɩɩ ho fãgadaar kpɩɛr, dɩ wɩ tʋʋ yʋʋra,
41015018	sa ma dɩ wa-n fʋɔrʋʋ ayɩ: Juifi fãgadaar gba fʋɔrɛ.
41015019	Sɩ dɩ wa-n bɩɩrʋʋ yʋʋ na ɓalʋʋ dɩ wa-n cɩɩrnanaa nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ, sɩ dɩ wɩ gburõku na fʋɔrʋʋ.
41015020	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ maanʋʋnɩ pɩ, wɩ thʋbʋʋrɛ kẽkẽ sɩɛ sa bir tʋʋ ɔɔ kẽkẽ sa kpaa thena wɩ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.
41015021	Kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a the lɔɔ da-n kɔ̃, dɩ wɩ kɔɔ cʋgʋʋ na fãga dɩ gba Jejuu kʋkʋ thɩr a heen; ɔɔ i n dʋɔn Sɩmɔ̃, Sɩrɛn dɩɩra a the, Alesãdɩɩr na Rufusii thɩ gɩ.
41015022	Dɩ wɩ kpa Jeju a jalna paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Gɔlgɔta, kɩrʋ dʋɔn Yʋ khubu.
41015023	Dɩ wɩ haarɛ taanɩkɛ nyanyaananɩ thɩɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ mɩɩr, sɩ a kɔɔ bor.
41015024	Agɩpɩ wɩ gbaarɛ a kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra, sa gba ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ a tɩnɛ na lɩ lɩr wɩ jɩ ntɛɛkɛ na 'lɛnɩ.
41015025	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpaanɩ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra, khɛ yɔ kpãa bɔɔ gɩ kɔɔ do.
41015026	Kherereekɛ n nɛnanɩ ɔɔ so heen kɩr ha gɩrɛ, gɩ sor: Juifi fãgadaar gɩ.
41015027	Wɩ kɔɔ kpar dakha yu hɔ̃hɔla yenyɔ dapaale, bɩɛl ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra, bɩɛl ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɩlana.
41015028	[Mɛ̃ gɩrɛɛkɛ kherenenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Wɩ kɔɔ theruure a ɓã puu cʋʋdarara” dã otirə.]
41015029	Wɩrɛ n thɛnɩ le sɩ wa-n ka wɩ-n nɩɩrʋʋrɛ sɩ dɩ wɩ didiə yʋʋ sɩ na so: Mee fɩ kɔɔ yɩ fa wɩɛrɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ sɩ fɩ bir fɩ mɩ wire balãther;
41015030	taa afɩbara a gbuno kʋkʋ thɩrʋra bɛɛ.
41015031	Mɛ̃ dakha bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara n ɓoɓororaa awɩ ha dɩ wa-n so aa: A kɔɔ taarɛ wɩ̃ tibil sɩ aa puno na taa dɩbara ga.
41015032	Dɔ ɔrkɛ dɔnɩ Kirisiti, Ɩjɩrayɛl fãgadaar n gbũ nɛnɛ̃ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra sɩ tor yire sɩ pɛr haar. Wɩrɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpanaanɩ kha n nɩɩrʋʋrɛ dakha wer.
41015033	A wire ʋlkha dɩɩ koo kɔɔ birəre tĩtĩtĩ a dana dʋɔr bɔɔ.
41015034	Dɩ dʋɔr bɔɔ, Jeju kɔɔ hulene nɔ khɩɩr aa: Eloyɩ, Eloyɩ, lama sabakɩtanɩ; kɩrʋ dʋɔn: Ɩ̃ Thãgba, ɩ̃ Thãgba mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fɩ bo mɩ faa?
41015035	Sɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ hanɩle dɩ wa-n nɩɛ, wɩ sor: Nɩ hɩnɛ, Elɩ Thãgbaa bobon a-n we.
41015036	Dɩ tibil bɩɛl wɛrra car a gba tabɩhʋɛ a mʋʋ ta ƴʋɔna, a gar jʋmuunə a 'laaraa a yɔ, sa so: Nɩ dɔ sɩ hɩɩn ado Elɩra na ɩnɛ na cʋgʋʋ dɩ na gbũ.
41015037	Sɩ Jeju hulene nɔ kheu sa khi.
41015038	Dɩ kẽkẽ nɩɩkɛ hanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna kɔɔ fʋrɛ ƴũ a ɓəər yenyɔ a ba dana thɩɩ.
41015039	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ jɩlɛnɩ Jejuu ƴɛra yɩnɩ khi caale Jeju khini, a sor: Sobɔr gɩ, Thãgbaa Bikuun kuunikɛ do ger.
41015040	Khɛrasɔ kɔɔ hale dakha a 'laa yɩɛ; Marɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Magɩdala dɩɩra, Salome, nakha Marɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Jakɩ diine na Jojɩɩ nɩ, wɩrɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ har khɛraalee thɩ̃thɩɩn.
41015041	Wɛr n kɔɔ kpaanɛ Jejura dɩ wa-n buluu ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ hanɩ Galile, na wɩ̃ khɛrsɔ bərəəmkɛ n kɔɔ jalanaanɩ kha Jerujalɛm kɔɔ hale wer.
41015042	Dɩɩ 'lire dʋɔrɛ sɩ dɩɩ do gbɛbɩ wire gɩ, a thɩɛna gaa gɛr dʋɔn hɩɩr wi dɛɛsɩ wire.
41015043	Jojɛfɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Arɩmate kɔɔ pɔr, ɔr dʋɔn tibilikɛ dɔnɩ so gʋʋr kɔ̃tɩn dakha kɛ wɩ-n cʋnɩ, ɔɔ thɛthɛ dakha n pɩɛrɛ bɔɔkɛ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do na ɩnɩ; a kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a pɛr kũu fɩlɛ sa jal Pɩlatɩɩ pa a bɩɛlaa a ha nɩ Jejuu for.
41015044	Sɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ Pɩlatɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a nɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do a 'lire khir, dɩ mɛ̃ a we sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ a bulee ado Jeju kɔɔ mãa khir.
41015045	Mɔ̃ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ mɩɛɛnɩ, gɛr a harɔ Jojɛfɩ hʋɛ dɩ gba Jejuu for.
41015046	Dɩ Jojɛfɩ ther kẽkẽ bulo ɓʋ̃ɔ, sa gbũ Jejuu for a par kɩ̃kɩɩnna, sa dʋʋ kaaraakɛ wɩ kɔɔ thelnɩ gɔ̃gʋɔna, agɩpɩ dɩ kpuro bokaar a khaanna ka nʋɔ.
41015047	Sɩ Marɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Magɩdala na Marɩ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ Jojɩɩ nɩ kɔɔ hɩɩnɛ ka wɩ kɔɔ pɩɛnɩ.
41016001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ hɩɩr wire kanɩ pɩ, Marɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Magɩdala, Salome, na Marɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Jakɩɩ nɩ kɔɔ ther niinikɛ n hʋnanɩ daʋ, a jalna wɩ thir Jejuu forra.
41016002	Sɩ duuro phiphi wire makonyɔɔ caca wi, wɩ kɔɔ jaal kaara wi phã bɔɔ.
41016003	Sɩ wɩ-n mɩɩrɛ khasɔ ayɩ: Amɛ na ba kpurone sar bokaar ka nʋɔra na faa ya fɛ?
41016004	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ gbanɩ wɩ hɩɩn, wɩ yɩrɛ bokaar dɩɩ kpuro a khokhɩa, sɩ ga do bokaar gɩ a wabɩ kpãkpalã ga.
41016005	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ lʋʋn kaʋ a yɩ daɓolbir dɩ too mɔ̃ wa-n lonɩ a pɛr nyɔ̃bɔɔ, a to kẽkẽ gbã bulo, dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɛr.
41016006	Sɩ a so warɛ: Na-n do nʋɔ n kpaa na'; mee Najarɛtɩ Jejuukɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpanɩ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra nɩ-n ƴaal. A ɩɩrɛ a the khirera, aa ha kɛka'; nɩ yɛ ka wɩ kɔɔ pɩɛnɩ.
41016007	Sɩ nɩ jala a sɔ ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara nakha Pɩɛrra ayɛ: A kʋʋl nɛr ƴɩɛ da-n jal Galile, dɩ le na yɩɩ mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ so narnɩ.
41016008	Dɩ mɛ̃ khɛraale kɔɔ the kaʋ a caalɛ gɩdonɩ nʋɔ kpaa wɛr dɩ wa-n jẽ, sɩ wa kɔɔ so tibillə thɩ̃a', gɩdonɩ maar fʋlɛnɛ wɩ.
41016009	[Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ khirera pɩ, wire makonyɔɔ caca wi duuro phiphi, Magɩdala Marɩɩkɛ a kɔɔ weeronɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbii makonyɔ a faa a kɔɔ nɩna dɩbara ɓo.
41016010	Ɔr kɔɔ jala a mɩɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ hanɩ wɩrɛraakɛ n kɔɔ hananɩ kha Jeju, kɛ n bɩɛnnɩ dɩ wa-n khɩɩna.
41016011	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ Jeju hananɛ yire dɩ ɩnɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ yɩɩ, wa kɔɔ pɛr haara'.
41016012	Agɩpɩ tɩbɩla yenyɔ wɛrra kɔɔ ha hʋɛra dɩ wa-n jal kõgoso, dɩ Jeju kɔɔ nɩna wɩ dɩbara a ha kpɩɩ.
41016013	Dɩ wɛr dakha kɔɔ jaal a mɩɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ sɛnɩ, sɩ wa kɔɔ pɛr haar dakha wera'.
41016014	A gele pɩ, a kɔɔ nɩnanɛ ɔɔbara kpãkpãadara yʋɔr bɩɛl, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ dɩko kho paar, a kɔɔ phaan wɛr awɩ ha pɛ ɓɔrra na mɔ̃kɛ awɩda khɩɩrnɩ, gɩdonɩ wa kɔɔ pɛr wɩrɛɛkɛ yɩɛnɩ na yireeda haara'.
41016015	Agɩpɩ a so warɛ: Nɩ jala thɩɩra fɛʋ a na mɩa Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ.
41016016	Ʋrɛɛkɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar dɩ wa kpɛgʋʋ nyʋɔnɔ a na 'lɛr taarɛ, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haara', sor na heenuune.
41016017	Nɩ yɛ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ jenaakɛ na kpaanɛnɩ wɩrɛraakɛ na-n pɩɛrnɩ haar: Wa gbaar ɩ̃ i wa-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ, wa-n mɩɩrɛ thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩsɔ;
41016018	wa fʋrɛ siisɔ; a wɩ yɔ kpalʋ, ga pɛ war thɩlkɩɩr fɩɩʋraka'; wa dɛɛnɛ khodarara nyɛ̃ɛ dɩ wa kpɛɛ.
41016019	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩnɩ pɩ, Thãgba kɔɔ khəsuure da-n jʋʋn Thãgbaa dʋɔ a too ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra.
41016020	Dɩ kpãkpãadara jaal dɩ wa-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ paar fɛʋ, dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn n dona wɛr kha thɔma, dɩ gba jenaakɛ n kpaanɛnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩra da-n nɩna dɩ sobɔr gɩ do.]
42001001	Tιbιl jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ 'lire dʋʋr bʋɔ, a khere thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ cʋɛnι asι thɩ̃thιιn,
42001002	mɔ̃kɛ tιbιlaakɛ dɔnι sobɔ so jιdara gbanι mιι sι dιι ha, kɛ dɔnι wιrɛ kɔɔ yɛ gιnι na yire dιι fʋna ga fʋ bɔɔ, wι dor dakha Thãgbaa thιmιι mιιdara.
42001003	Mɛrɛ dakha, mι jιɛ 'lo bɔɔbɔɔ, a jι mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛlera kɔɔ ιιrnι fʋ paarrakɛ kɛkɛkɛ, dι mι yιɛrɛ dιι do gι bɔrɛ dι ɩ̃ khere gιrɛ kpa kha kpa kha, dι ma-n mιɛ fι, fɛr Teofιl bʋɔ,
42001004	fι puno fι jιι jι, dι sobɔr dιιrɛɛlera fι kɔɔ 'lɛnι do.
42001005	Dabɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdι donι fãgadaar Jude dιιra, Thãgbaa bonι jidaar bιɛl kɔɔ hale wι-n wenι Jakarι, Abιaa too gι. Ɔɔ khɛr, kɛ wι-n wenι Elijabɛtι, dɔ Aarɔ̃ɔkɛ dɔnι gbõdaarι məl.
42001006	Dι wɛr yenyɔ fɛʋ dor tιbιlaakɛ saranι Thãgbaa ƴɛra. Dι wι-n hιιnɛ Kɔ̃tιnι jɔfʋsɔ na ɔɔ so fɛʋ, wa hana so paara'.
42001007	Sι wa hana bιsaana', gιdonι Elijabɛtι dor khɛr kʋ̃bʋʋ, wɛr yenyɔ fɛʋ tιnɛ.
42001008	Dι wi bιɛl, Jakarι n dor ɔɔ bonι ji thɔ̃ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, gιdonι ɔɔ too dea mɛ̃.
42001009	Mɔ̃kɛ bonι jidara n cʋʋnι, wι lιrɛ lιι dιι do ɔɔda gι, dι na lõ Kɔ̃tιnι fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tιιna an thii thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnanι daʋ.
42001010	Sι tibil jɔ derre phiilo, dι wa-n bιɛl Thãgba, dabɔɔkɛ Jakarι n thiini thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnanι daʋ.
42001011	Le Kɔ̃tιnι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bιɛl the Jakarιra a jιιl nyɔ̃bɔɔra, paarιkɛ wι-n thiini thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnanι daʋ.
42001012	A Jakarι yιι, haar fuguure dι maar fʋʋ.
42001013	Sι Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu sʋʋraa ayι: Jakarι, fa-n do maar n fʋ fa', gιdonι Thãgba ture afι bιɛl. Afι khɛr Elijabɛtι na kʋɔn kũubir, dι fa dʋʋ ire Jã.
42001014	A na do farɛ dadaa na kãkadaa, dι daʋ na fʋrɛ tibil jɔjʋɔ ɔɔ kɔna.
42001015	Gιdonι a na dor tibil kɔ̃tɩ̃ι Kɔ̃tιnι ƴɛra, a na yɔ dιvɛ̃ dι ta khaa ga, a na hinəne Thu Phuu dabɔɔkɛrakɛ a hanι ɔɔ nιι kɔ̃lora.
42001016	Dι ɔr na cʋɛ Ɩjιrayɛl bιsana jɔɔjɔɔ, dι wa kɛr na bir Kɔ̃tιn awι Thãgbara.
42001017	Dι ɔr na kʋlɛ Kirisiti ƴιɛ, a hanana Elι Thãgbaa bobonι thu ca na ɔɔ puno, a cʋʋna thɛɛ ha gι bir gι ha awι bιsãsɔra, sɩ a kpa nũ nʋʋrdara a pɛr wɩ hana tɩɩ saraa kpɛsɛ, gɩ do mɛ̃ a gbɛbɩ tɩbɩla dɩ wɩ too Kɔ̃tɩnɩ too.
42001018	Dɩ Jakarɩ bule Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurə: Mɔ̃ ma jɩ dɩ sobɔr thɩ̃ɛɛlera na do, gɩdonɩ mɩ tɩnɛ dɩ ɩ̃ khɛr dakha tɩ̃?
42001019	Dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bir birsee: Mɛr dʋɔn Gabɩrɩɛlɩkɛ n jɩlɛnɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra. A thɔ̃ mɛr ayɩ, ɩ̃ sɔ far a mɩana fɩ dakha tutugo bʋɔɔkɛra.
42001020	Dɩ hɩnɛ, gɩdonɩ fa kɔɔ pɛr haar ɩ̃ thιmιιsɔraakɛ na dananι a ga bɔ dã ga, fa dor nɔ madaar, fa puno a na mιι thιmιιra' phaphapha gι dana wireekɛ gιrɛɛkɛra na danι.
42001021	Sι tιbιla har dι wa-n pιɛr Jakarι, dι nʋɔ kpaa wɛr mɔ̃ a-n pʋɔrnι le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιnɔ.
42001022	Sι ɔbɔɔkɛ Jakarι thenι aa-n puno na mιιna wι thιmιιra'. Dι mɛ̃ wι jι thɩ̃ɛ a yι le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιnɔ. Dι a mar da-n mιιna wι na nyɛ̃be, dιι do nɔ marra a toona thalera.
42001023	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ Jakarιι thɔ̃ do wi pιnι, a bire kɔ̃ ɔɔ cɔ.
42001024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ ga toonι gbe, dιι do ɔɔ khɛr Elijabɛtι hananɛ pɛmɛr da-n toona cɔ haar dιι cʋʋna pora yemɔι, sι dι so ayι:
42001025	Hιnɛ gιrɛɛkɛ Kɔ̃tιn cʋʋ marnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a hɩɩn mɩnɩ sa ti gɩrɛɛkɛ dɔ marnɩ yicuru tɩbɩlala.
42001026	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Elijabɛtɩ hananɩ pɛmɛr dɩɩ cʋʋ pora maadõ, Thãgba bire thɔ̃ ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu Gabɩrɩɛl Galile, dɩ bɩɛllakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Najarɛtɩ,
42001027	khɛ biireraakɛ na jɛnɩ kuun pa'. Sɩ a hananɛ wɛdaar, kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jojɛfɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Davɩdɩɩ tibil. Dɩ khɛ biireelee irə n dʋɔn Marɩ.
42001028	Le Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu pɔ Marɩɩ pa, a sʋʋraa: Mι fʋɔr fɛr, fɛrɛɛkɛ Thãgba jιnι bʋɔra, Kɔ̃tιn har kha na fɛrɛ.
42001029	Sι mɔ̃kɛ Marι nιɛnι ga thιmιιle, haar fuguure ka dι bule ɔɔbara: Anye dɔ fʋɔr caakɛɛ kιr ya fɛ?
42001030	Dι Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu sʋʋraa: Marι, fa-n do maar n fʋ fa', gιdonι Thãgba jɩɛn fι bʋɔra.
42001031	Dι hιnɛ, fa hananɛ pɛmɛr a na kɔ̃ kũubir a na dʋʋ ire Jeju.
42001032	A na dor tibil kɔ̃tɩ̃ι, dι ɔɔ i na-n dɔ Kəkəədaarι Bikuun, dι Kɔ̃tιn Thãgba na haarɛ ɔɔ mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃ Davιdιι fãga too pa.
42001033	Dι mɛ̃ a na do fãgadaar khorr Jakɔbιι toora, dι ɔɔ fãgadaar do na hana khu paara'.
42001034	Dι Marι so Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurə: Mɔ̃ ga do sι na ha thale gιdonι ma jι kuun pa?
42001035	Dι Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu birsee: Thu Phuu na ιna na ha far, dι Kəkəədaar na ɔɔ fãga na kɛɛ farɛ ιtιιr. Gɛr gι bιsaanιkɛ fa kɔnι, wa-n wιιrɛ daphuu, Thãgbaa Bikuun.
42001036	Dι hιnɛ, Elijabɛtι afι tibil, a hananɛ pɛmɛr dakha ɔɔ tɩ̃ bɔra, dι kũubir a na kɔ̃, ɔrkɛ wι-n kɔɔ wenι khɛr kʋ̃bʋʋ hana gɛr pora maadõ gι cʋʋ nɛnɛ̃.
42001037	Gιdonι thɩ̃ bιɛl na hale kpιιkɛ Thãgba na-n punonaa ga.
42001038	Dι Marι birsee: Hιnɛ, mι dor Kɔ̃tιnι thɔ̃daar, dɔ gι dã mι mɔ̃kɛra fι sonι. Dι Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu fagʋʋ sa jal.
42001039	Dawiilera Marι ιιr a gba hʋɛ na phananɛ, da-n jal gɔ̃gɔ̃ khʋra Juda dι bιɛlla,
42001040	a lõ Jakarιι cɔ a fʋɔr Ehjabɛtι.
42001041	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ Elijabɛtι nιɛnι Marιι fʋɔr, ɔɔ bi ubire le ɔɔ kɔ̃lora, dι Elijabɛtι hinə Thu Phuu,
42001042	a hulẽ na nɔ kheu ayι: Thãgba bɔna fɛr a jɔ khɛra fɛʋ, dι biilera afι kɔ̃lora 'lɛr bɔnanɛ.
42001043	Mɔ̃ gι fʋ sι ɩ̃ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ι nι ɩ̃ a yι mι?
42001044	Gιdonι hιnɛ, dapaara afι fʋɔr lõ mιnι nũ kaar, ɩ̃ bi ubire na kãkar kɛ ɩ̃ kɔ̃lora.
42001045	Gι da fɛrkɛra pιɛrnι haar, gιdonι gιrɛ thɛnι Kɔ̃tιnι pa dι wι mιι fι, ga daan oti.
42001046	Dι Marι so ayι: Ɩ̃ ha n khιιrɛ Kɔ̃tιn,
42001047	dι ɩ̃ ha na-n kãka Thãgba ɩ̃ Taadaarra,
42001048	gιdonι a hιιnɛ ɔɔ hɛlɛlɛ thɔ̃daar khɛr. Gιdonι hιnɛ, a fʋna nɛnɛ̃kɛ, thɩ kɔ̃ caar fɛʋ na so marɛ anayι, Thãgba bɔna mɛr.
42001049	Gιdonι Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ Punodaar cʋʋ marɛ thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩna; dι ɔɔ i n dʋɔn daphuu.
42001050	Dɔ ɔɔ bɔ dona n hale wιrɛraakɛ n maanɛɛnι məlle wo məllela fɛʋ.
42001051	A nιnanɛ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ fãga nyɔ̃ hanι, a bɩ̃bιlanɛ wιrɛɛkɛ hananι i ƴaal kpιɛrɛsɔ haarra.
42001052	A tɔr fãgadara awι fãga too para kpɛɛ, sa cʋʋ hɛlɛlɛ fιldara dι wι pal ιιr.
42001053	A cʋʋrɛ kɔmɛdara dɩ wɩ hi na thɩ̃ bʋɔ, sa faa lɛ̃lɛ na nyɛ̃ biire dɩ wɩ jal.
42001054	A bulle Ɩjɩrayɛl ɔɔ thɔ̃daar, gɩdonɩ ɔɔ bɔ donana a jɩna
42001055	Abɩraham na ɔɔ məlsɔ khorr, mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ sonɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔra.
42001056	Dɩ Marɩ too nakha Elijabɛtɩ pora yẽthersɔ. Agɩpɩ dɩ kɛr bir kɔ̃ ɔɔ cɔ.
42001057	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ Elijabɛtιι bi kɔ̃ bɔ danι, a kʋɔn kũubir.
42001058	A Elijabɛtιι cɔ khudara na ɔɔ toosɔ nιɛ dι Kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ donaanɛ bʋɔ dιι kar, wι-n kãkarɛ kha na ɔr.
42001059	Dι wire makõther wirera, wι pɔr a kur biile khʋ̃ʋ, sa ƴaal wι haa ire Jakarι, kɛ dɔnι ɔɔ thιι irə wo.
42001060	Sι ɔɔ nι so: Kpei, Jã wa-n wιι.
42001061	Dι wι sʋʋraa: Tibil na hale afι toora a hana ire thala';
42001062	sa mιιna ɔɔ thι nyɛ̃be wι hιιn mɔ̃kɛ a-n ƴaalnι a na-n wιι.
42001063	Dι Jakarι bιɛl sɛbɛ a khere pɛr ayι: Jã wa-n wιι. Dι nʋɔ kpaa wι fɛʋ.
42001064	Dι dapaara Jakarιι nɔ khɛr, dι delẽbire lιmι dι puno wo da-n mιι thιmιa, da-n khιιna Thãgba.
42001065	Dι maar fʋlɛ cɔ khudara fɛʋ, dι Jude gɔ̃gɔ̃ dιdara fɛʋ kɔɔ mιιrɛ kha ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera.
42001066	Dι wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ nιɛnɛnι thɩmɩɩrɩle, wι fʋ gɛr le awι bιnɔ sι wa-n so aa: Dι mɔ̃ biilera na ha ya fɛ? Sι Kɔ̃tιnι nyɔ̃ kɔɔ kɛɛraarɛ.
42001067	Dι ɔɔ thι Jakarι hinə Thu Phuu, a ma da-n ti Thãgba tukιrʋ thakɛ ayι:
42001068	Kɔ̃tιnιkɛ dɔnι Ɩjιrayɛl Thãgba hιna khιιrɛ, gιdonι a ιnɛ a kher ɔɔ too sa birse wi.
42001069	A pɛ sarɛ Taadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ι ɔɔ thɔ̃daar Davιdιι toora,
42001070	mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ mιιnι dιι the ɔɔ bobon phusɔɔ nɔɔ kɛkɛkɛ;
42001071	taarɛ gι dι ga-n taa sι asι sodarara, na wιrɛraakɛ fɛʋ n laarɛ sιnιι nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
42001072	Mɛ̃ a kɔɔ dona asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ bʋɔ, a jɩnana ɔɔ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ phu.
42001073	Gɛr dʋɔn nʋɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ sonɩ na asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abɩraham,
42001074	dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba na ha sɩ fãga, ɔbɔɔkɛ a na taa sɩnɩ asɩ sodaraa nyɔ̃kɔɔ na pɩ, sa-n dʋʋraa thɔma na 'lar,
42001075	na phur, na fɩl sarʋ ɔɔ ƴɛra wire fɛʋ asɩ yi hanana.
42001076	Sɩ fɛrɛ bɩsã buu, wa we fer Kəkəədaarɩ bobon, gɩdonɩ fɛr na kʋlɛ Kɔ̃tɩn ƴɩɛ, fa-n gbɛbɩrɩ ɔɔ hʋsʋnɔ.
42001077	Dɩ mɛ̃ a na nɩna ɔɔ too taa jɩɩr, dɩ ga ther awɩ sopugosɔɔ faara,
42001078	gɩdonɩ asɩ Thãgba hinəne bɔ donanɛ, gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ƴũu dahɩrɛ phã a ɩ̃ a kher sɩ;
42001079	a na-n hɩrɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ hanɩ dabirəra, na khi jəərera, a thɔɔ asɩ nɛ a na-n pɛ ha ie hʋɛra.
42001080	Dɩ bɩsaanna n khʋɔn, dɩ ɔɔ thu na-n 'lɛ fãga. Sɩ bəənnə a-n cɔ, phaphapha dɩɩ dana wireekɛ a nɩnanɩ ɔɔbara Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
42002001	Ɔbɔɔlera, Sejaar Ogusiti fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ kɔɔ 'laa jɔfʋ ayɩ, wɩ thera tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
42002002	Dɩ caca therreele kɔɔ har ɔbɔɔkɛ Kiriniyusi donɩ gobanɛr Siri dɩɩra.
42002003	Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ jaal wɩ ther wɩ awɩ dɩraakɛ wɩ thenɩ.
42002004	Dɩ Jojɛfɩ dakha kɛ thɛnɩ Galile Najarɛtɩ dɩɩra, a jaal Jude Davɩdɩɩ dɩraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Bɛtɩlɛhɛm, gɩdonɩ Davɩdɩɩ tibil gι a do ɔɔ ca.
42002005	A jaal dakha na Marι, ɔɔ wɛdaarιkɛ hananι pɛmɛr wι ther wι.
42002006	Dι mɔna wι hanιle, Marιι bi kɔ̃ bɔ daan,
42002007	dι kɔ̃ ɔɔ biir bi dι do kũubir, dι parʋʋ bibɔrɔ kɩ̃kιιn a pɛ bekolela, gιdonι phɩ̃ paar na hale kãkɛ kpakpala n cɔnι dι wa ha wa'.
42002008	Dι khuirəəle bana khedara hale hʋɔnɔ, dι wa-n bɛr awι banasɔ dιtιnɔ.
42002009	Dι le Kɔ̃tιnι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bιɛl the war, dι Kɔ̃tιnι carbara hιrɛrɛ a dii war. Dι maar fʋlɛ wι jɔɔ ka.
42002010	Dι Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuulera so warɛ ayι: Na-n do maar n fʋ na', gιdonι tutugo bʋɔ mι-n mιι nι kɛ na dɔnι da kɔ̃tɩ̃ι Ɩjιrayɛldarara fɛʋ.
42002011	Nĩkɛ nι 'lɛr Taadaar bιɛlιkɛ dʋɔnnι Kirisiti, Kɔ̃tιn gι, kɛ wι kɔnι Davιdιι dιra.
42002012	Dι gιrɛɛkɛ na dɔ narnι jιιn dʋɔn: Na yιrɛ bibɔrɔ, dι wa parʋʋ bibɔrɔ kɩ̃kιιn na pɛ bekolela.
42002013	Le dapaara ƴũ ko kena tə̃tə̃tə̃ the Thãgbaa dʋɔ a caan Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule, dι wa-n khιι kha Thãgba awι ha, dι wa-n sona aa:
42002014	Thãgbaa i n dʋbarɔ le thãgbara ƴũ pər, sι ha ιι n dɛɛnɛ tιbιlala thιιra, kɛ n lonaanι haar.
42002015	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔle faa wɩnɩ, sɩ wa-n bir Thãgbaa dʋɔ, bana khedaraale mɩɩrɛ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl ayɩ: Dɩ a mɛ̃ gɩ, nɩ ɩna sɩ jal phaphapha sɩ dã Bɛtɩlɛhɛm sɩ hɩɩn gɩrɛ dananɩ le, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛra Kɔ̃tɩn cʋʋ sɩnɩ dɩ sɩ jɩ.
42002016	Dɩ wɩ jaal khə̃khə̃ a ƴaal Marɩ, na Jojɛfɩ, na bibɔrɔɔle wɩ pɛnɩ bekolela a yɩ wɩ.
42002017	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ pɩ, wɩ gbaar thɩmɩa fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ bɩsã buudaraale a mɩɩ.
42002018	Dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ, nʋɔ kpaa wɛr bana khedaraa thɩmɩɩraale.
42002019	Sɩ Marɩ fʋrɛ ga thɩ̃sɔɔle fɛʋ ɔɔ bɩnɔ da-n kpɩɛrna gɩ.
42002020	Dɩ bana khedara kɛrrɛ a dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i dɩ wa-n birnə, dɩ wa-n khɩɩnaa dakha gɩrɛraakɛ fɛʋ wɩ nɩɛnɩ a torna yire, gɩdonɩ gɩ har mɔna Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuulera kɔɔ so warnɩ.
42002021	A wire makõther dã, wɩ kurre biile khʋ̃ʋ sɩ wa-n wɩɩ Jeju, ireekɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ 'laanɩ sɩ ɔɔ nɩ na hana ɔɔ pɛmɛ pa'.
42002022	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jojɛfɩ na Marɩɩ phʋɔl wi danɩ, mɔ̃kɛ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ hanɩ, wɩ gbaar Jeju a jalna Jerujalɛm wɩ ha Kɔ̃tɩn.
42002023	Gɩdonɩ mɛ̃ gɩ khere Kɔ̃tɩnɩ jɔfʋra ayɩ: “Caca kuuminə fɛʋʋkɛ wa kɔnɩ, Kɔ̃tɩnɩda wa do.”
42002024	Dɩ Jojɛfɩ na Marɩ 'laarɛ bonɩ jirrə, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ jɔfʋra, “kʋlãpuo yenyɔ agɩbo puusɛ̃ ɓɔla yenyɔ.”
42002025	Dɩ hɩnɛ, kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a hale Jerujalɛm dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Sɩmɛ̃ʋ. Kuunile dor tibil sarʋ, da-n cʋna Thãgba. A-n pιɛrɛ dakha ʋrɛɛkɛ Ɩjιrayɛl na 'lɛrɔnι taarɛ, dι Thu Phuu haaraa.
42002026	Thu Phuu kɔɔ khιιraarɛ gιrɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara, dɩ a na yɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ Kirisiti na yire sɩ na khi.
42002027	Dɩ Thu Phuurə thɔɔrɛ Sɩmɛ̃ʋ a jalna Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna. Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju bɩsã buulee thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ pɔnaanɩ, wɩ cʋʋnaa mɔ̃kɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ,
42002028	Sɩmɛ̃ʋ teguure a pɛ ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ sa khɩɩ Thãgba ayɩ:
42002029	Nɛnɛ̃kɛ Kɔ̃tɩn, sɛ afɩ thɔ̃daarra a kɔ̃ na ha ɩɩ mɔna fɩ kɔɔ sonɩ;
42002030	gɩdonɩ mɩ torre afɩ taara yire,
42002031	kɛ fɩ gbɛbɩnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra.
42002032	Taarɛɛle na dor dahɩrɛ a na hɩrɛ tibil caar fɛʋ, sɩ gɩ do i dʋbɩrɛ Ɩjɩrayɛl afɩ toora.
42002033	Nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ Jojɛfɩ na Marɩ gɩrɛraakɛ n mɩanɩ Jejura.
42002034	Dɩ Sɩmɛ̃ʋ bɩɛlɛ Thãgba a pɛ war, sa so Jejuu nɩ Marɩra ayɩ: Hɩnɛ, Thãgba cʋʋrɛ bɩsaanɩkɛ a dɔ ji paar na pal ɩɩr paar Ɩjɩrayɛldara jɔjʋɔra, na jɩɩnɩkɛ tɩbɩla na bananɩ;
42002035	dɩ mɛ̃ tibil jɔjʋɔɔ kpɩɛr gbulsɔ na yɩr, sɩ fe wer, khalghãa na gɔ fɛr haarra.
42002036	Thãgbaa bobon khɛ bιɛl gι, a kɔɔ hale dakha dι wa-n wιι An Panʋɛlι bikhɛr gι, a do Ajɛɛrι ca. A thʋnɛ tɩ̃ ka. A fʋna ɔɔ biir bɔɔ yɛna makonyɔ a kɔɔ cʋʋ na ɔɔ ko,
42002037	dι ɔɔ ko khi, sι dι too do khikhɛrʋ. Yɛna kpalanã yenã a hana, dι aa-n 'lee Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tιιna ga; Thãgbaa thɔ̃ a-n do dιtιnɔ na dιwιlʋ, dι li nʋɔ da-n bιɛlna Thãgba.
42002038	Dι bɔ bιɛllaalera, ɔr dakha pɔr da-n khιι Thãgba a mιιna Jejuuda tιbιla fɛʋraakɛ n pιɛrɛnι ʋrɛɛkɛ na birseneni Jerujalɛmdara.
42002039	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jojɛfι na Marι cʋʋnι thɩ̃ɛsɔ fɛʋ dιι pι, mɔ̃kɛ Kɔ̃tιnι jɔfʋ sonι, wι kɛrrɛ bir kɔ̃ Galile Najarɛtι awι dιra.
42002040	Dι bιsaan na-n khɔ̃ da-n 'lɛ fãga, dι ɔɔ kpɛsɛ dakha na-n jɔr da-n 'lɛna dakha Thãgbaa bɔna.
42002041	Bɔɔ fɛʋ ɔɔ thι na ɔɔ nι n jaal Jerujalɛm yɛna yɛna fɛtιιkɛ wι-n wenι Pakι.
42002042	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a hananι yɛna yʋɔr yenyɔ, wι jaal mɔ̃kɛ wι yιnι wa-n cʋɛ fɛtιra.
42002043	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ fɛtι pιnι dι wι bir dι wa-n kɔ̃, Jeju bιsaanιlera toore le Jerujalɛm, sɩ ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ na kɔɔ ja'.
42002044	Dɩ wɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ Jeju hale na awɩ kpakpaarsɔ, a ɩɩr waa dɩɩ na tɩ̃ɩ, sɩ wa-n ƴaalʋʋ awɩ too na awɩ jɩ jɩnaa pa.
42002045	Mɔ̃kɛ wa-n yɩɩna', wɩ kɛrrɛ bir Jerujalɛm dɩ wa-n jɩɩ ƴaalʋʋ.
42002046	A wire yẽther ka pɩ, wɩ yɩɩrɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna dɩ too dɩɩrdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn, da-n pɛ wɩ nũu da-n bulena wɩ thɩ̃ɛ.
42002047	Dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n kɔɔ pɩɛnɩ nũu, nʋɔ kpaa wɛr ɔɔ kpɛsɛra na mɔ̃ a-n birse wini.
42002048	A ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ yɩɩ, gɩ kpaa wɛr nʋɔ, dɩ ɔɔ nɩ bulee: Ɩ̃ bi ya, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fɩ cʋʋ sɩ thakɛ? Hɩnɛ, afɩ thɩ na mɛrɛ, sɩ kɔɔ ƴaal fɛr waa na dɛr.
42002049	Dɩ bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n kɔɔ ƴaal mɩ? Na jɩ dɩ gɩ teenanɛ dɩ ma cʋʋ ɩ̃ Thιι thɔ̃aa?
42002050	Sι wa jι thιmιιrιle a so warnι kιrʋa'.
42002051	Agιpι Jeju bire kɔ̃ nakha wɛr Najarɛtι dιιra da-n nι wι nũu. Dι ɔɔ nι fʋrɛ thιmιaale fɛʋ ɔɔ bιnɔ.
42002052	Sι Jeju n khʋɔn dι ɔɔ kpɛsɛ na-n pɛr, da-n da Thãgba haar na tιbιla.
42003001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Tɩbɛɛr Sejaar kɔɔ donɩ fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dɩ ga cʋʋ yɛna yʋɔr yemɔɩ, ga bɔɔlera Pɔ̃sɩ Pɩlatɩ do dakha gobanɛr Jude dɩɩra, sɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ do fãgadaar buu Galile dɩɩra, dɩ ɔɔ õkuun Filipi do Ituredara na Tɩrakonɩtɩdaraa fãgadaar bu, sɩ dɩ Lɩjanɩasɩ do Abɩlɛndaraa fãgadaar bu;
42003002	dɩ ɔbɔɔlera dakha An na Kaɩfɩ do gbõdara, gɛr Thãgba mɩɩna Jã, Jakarɩɩ bikuun, bəənnə.
42003003	Dɩ a jaal da-n kpaar dɩɩ fɛʋ Jʋrdɛ̃ khʋra, da-n so tɩbɩlala aa: Nɩ deba haar sa 'lɛ yɔ kpɛɛrɛ, sɩ Thãgba n faa anɩ sopugosɔ.
42003004	Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩɩdaakɛ a kɔɔ kherenɩ ɔɔ sɛbɛra dana mɛ̃ ayɩ. “Tibil wire gɩ dɩ ga-n hulẽ bəənnə ayɩ: Na-n gbɛbɩrɛ hʋɛ Kɔ̃tɩnna, na-n wɛbɩrɛ ɔɔ hʋ bisɔ gɩ pɔlɔ.
42003005	Bɛlɛ̃ɛ fɛʋ na hire, dɩ gɔ̃gɔ̃ kɔ̃tɩna na gɔ̃gɔ̃ biisɔ fɛʋ na yɩɩrɛ na mãkha na thɩɩ. Gɩrɛɛkɛ gõgolonenɩ ga bire na telẽ, dɩ hʋɛsɔɔkɛ hanɩ yara yara ga pɔlɔlɛ.
42003006	Dɩ tibil caar fɛʋ na yɩrɛ taarɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara.”
42003007	Sɩ Jana n sor tibil jɔraale n pʋɔraanɩ wɩ kpɛɛ nyʋɔnɔ dɩ yɩ: Nɛr sikori bisɔ, amɛ sɔ nar nɩ fuo Thãgbaa nĩkhirəəkɛ na ɩnanɩ?
42003008	A mɛ̃ gɩ na-n sɛ beekɛ n nɛnanɩ anɩ ha debi, sɩ na-n too na so le anɩ bɩnɔ ayɩ, Abɩraham dʋɔn anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tã'. Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ: Bokanaakɛrakɛ Thãgba punone a cʋʋ gɩ dɩ gɩ debi a do bɩsana Abɩrahamna.
42003009	Dɩrakɛ kpãkpo 'lire leere thɩr nɛ kuur leere. Dɩ thɩr wo thɩrʋʋkɛ na-n sɛnɩ bi bʋɔa', wa kuur ger na dʋna dɔɔra.
42003010	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle bulee aa: Dɩ a gɩ ha thale, mɔ̃ sa do?
42003011	Dɩ birse wi: Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ kẽkena yenyɔ, a te bɩɛl hana ʋrɛɛkɛ na hana gɩna'; dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ dɩkor, dɔ a cʋʋna ɔmɛna dakha.
42003012	Dɩ war gbadaraakɛ pʋɔnnɩ wɩ kpɛɛ nyʋɔnɔ dakha, wɩ bulele Jã: Dɩɩrdaar, dɩ mɔ̃ sa do?
42003013	Dɩ so war: Na-n taa tɩbɩlala thɩ̃ɛ gɩ kãasɩ gɩrɛraakɛ wɩ pɛrna'.
42003014	Dɩ sɔrasɛsɔ dakha bulee: Sɩ sɛrɛ, mɔ̃ sa do? Dɩ birse wi: Na-n tagɩrɩ tibillə thɩ̃ɛ na fãga bɩa', agɩbo na-n pɛ war so khɩa', sɩ nɩ dɔ gɩrɛ wɩ-n lɩmɩ nɩnɩ na-n da nar.
42003015	Mɔ̃kɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n pɛnɩ nũu dɩ wa-n kpɩɛr awɩ hara, Jã ba dʋɔn Kirisiti yaa,
42003016	Jã so warɛ fɛʋ ayɩ: Me wer nyʋɔnɔ mɩ-n kpɛɛ nɩ, sɩ tibil bɩɛl na ɩnɛ kɛ hananɩ fãga a jɔ mɩ, dɩ ma hɩɩrʋʋrakɛ a na thʋbʋʋ nɛfaa pɛ̃a'. Ɔr, Thu Phuurə na dɔɔra a na kpɛɛ nɩ.
42003017	Dɩ jʋ jɛ nyɔ̃kpʋʋn hale dι fʋrɔ ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ. A na jɛr jɔ a gba jʋ be a pɛ ɔɔ thʋ̃ bιnɔ, sι a thii laagbee dɔɔraakɛ na dɔnι thɩ̃ khiirnənə'.
42003018	Thale Jã n kɔɔ mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ tɩbɩlala nakha thɩmɩɩ ƴɩrɛ wo na bulo wini.
42003019	Sɩ gɩdonɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar buu kɔɔ gbaar ɔɔ õkuuni khɛr Ɛrɔdɩadɩ, Jã phaanʋʋnɛ ga phaan, na gɩ̃ sopugo jɔjɔraakɛ fɛʋ Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ.
42003020	Ɛrɔɔdɩ cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ puuro ka, sɩ gɩrɛ puuroni a jɔrakɛ dʋɔn mɔ̃ a fʋnɩ Jã a to khaɩra.
42003021	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jã kɔɔ kpɛɛnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ nyʋɔnɔ na pɩ, a kɔɔ kpɛɛrɛ Jeju dakha nyʋɔnɔ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju hanɩ da-n bɩɛl Thãgba, thãgbara ƴũ phubire.
42003022	Dɩ Thu Phuu gbũ puusɛ̃ khaa gbelẽ gbelẽ a lʋʋnaa. Dɩ le nʋɔ the thãgbara ƴũ ayɩ: Fɛr dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, fɩ lõ mer haar kpɛ.
42003023	Jeju kɔɔ hananɛ yɛna dɩɩ thɔɔ kpelẽ yʋɔrsɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a fʋnɩ ɔɔ thɔ̃. Dɩ tɩbɩla n kpɩɛrɛ Jojɛfɩɩ bikuun a do na Elɩɩ bikuun,
42003024	Matatɩɩ bikuun, Levɩɩ bikuun, Mɛlkɩɩ bikuun, Janaɩɩ bikuun, Jojɛfɩɩ bikuun,
42003025	Matatɩasɩɩ bikuun, Amɔsɩɩ bikuun, Nahʋmɩ bikuun, Esɩlɩɩ bikuun, Nagaɩɩ bikuun,
42003026	Matɩɩ bikuun, Matatɩasɩɩ bikuun, Semeɩɩ bikuun, Jojɛkɩɩ bikuun, Jodaa bikuun,
42003027	Joanãa bikuun, Rejaa bikuun, Jorobabɛlɩ bikuun, Salatɩɛlɩ bikuun, Nerɩɩ bikuun,
42003028	Mɛlkɩɩ bikuun, Adɩɩ bikuun, Kosamɩ bikuun, Ɛlmadamɩ bikuun, Ɛrɩ bikuun,
42003029	Jejuu bikuun, Elɩɛjɛɛrɩ bikuun, Jorɩmɩ bikuun, Matatɩɩ bikuun, Levɩɩ bikuun,
42003030	Sɩmɛ̃ʋʋ bikuun, Judaa bikuun, Jojɛfɩɩ bikuun, Jonamɩ bikuun, Elɩakɩmɩ bikuun,
42003031	Meleaa bikuun, Menaa bikuun, Matataa bikuun, Natãa bikuun, Davɩdɩɩ bikuun,
42003032	Ɩjaɩɩ bikuun, Jobɛɛdɩɩ bikuun, Boajɩɩ bikuun, Salomɔ̃ɔ bikuun, Nasɔ̃ɔ bikuun,
42003033	Amɩnadabɩɩ bikuun, Adɩmɛ̃ɛ bikuun, Arnɩɩ bikuun, Ɛsɩrɔmɩ bikuun, Farɛsɩɩ bikuun, Judaa bikuun,
42003034	Jakɔbɩɩ bikuun, Ɩjakɩɩ bikuun, Abɩrahamɩ bikuun, Taraa bikuun, Nakɔɔrɩ bikuun,
42003035	Serukii bikuun, Ragoo bikuun, Falɛkɩɩ bikuun, Ebɛɛrɩ bikuun, Salaa bikuun,
42003036	Kaɩnamɩ bikuun, Arfasaadɩɩ bikuun, Sɛmɩ bikuun, Noee bikuun, Lamɛkɩɩ bikuun,
42003037	Matujalaa bikuun, Enɔkɩɩ bikuun, Jarɛɛdɩɩ bikuun, Malelɛlɩ bikuun, Kaɩnãa bikuun,
42003038	Enɔsɩɩ bikuun, Sɛtɩɩ bikuun, Adãa bikuun, na Thãgbaa bikuun a do.
42004001	A Jeju hinə Thu Phuu, a ther Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩrɔ, dɩ Thu Phuu thɔgʋʋ a jalna bəənnə.
42004002	Le Satã fifiləə a cʋʋna wire kpalanyɔ. Dɩ Jeju na kɔɔ kho dɩkor ga wisɔraala'; a ga wiile ka pɩ kɔmɛr fʋʋrɛ.
42004003	Dɩ le Satã sʋʋraa aa: Ado fɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun, sɔ bokaarraakɛ gɩ debi gɩ do dɩkor.
42004004	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Ga do dɩkor dɩbara na hana tibil yirə'.”
42004005	Dɩ Satã kpaa a jʋʋnna ƴũ, a nɩɩraa dapaara fãgadaar dɩɩsɔ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ thɩɩra,
42004006	sa sʋʋraa: Fɛr ma ha fãga fãgadaar dɩɩsɔraakɛ fɛʋ na awɩ nyɔ̃kor bɔ, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ ha mɛr, dɩ ma har ntɛɛkɛ mɩ pɛrnɩ haar ɩ̃ ha.
42004007	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ado fa gburõkure na fʋɔr mɩ, afɩda ga do fɛʋ.
42004008	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Gι kherere ayɩ: “Kɔ̃tɩn, afɩ Thãgba fa fʋɔr, dɩ ɔrra dιbara fa doro thɔma.”
42004009	Dɩ Satana kpaa wo, a jalna Jerujalɛm a jʋʋnna Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna ƴũ, sa sʋʋraa: Ado fɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun, bɩna kɩɛr a je thʋnɔ, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere ayɩ:
42004010	“A na pɛrɛ ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ dɩ wa hɩɩn fɩ”
42004011	dɩ “wa tɛ fɛr, agado mã' fa ber nɔɔ bokaarra.”
42004012	Sɩ Jeju birsee: Gɩ kherere ayɩ: “Fa-n fifilə Kɔ̃tɩn afɩ Thãgba a hɩɩna'.”
42004013	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Satã kɔɔ fifiləəni na fɩlɛ fɛʋʋle pɩ, a fagʋʋrɛ phaphapha a yɩ hʋ kpɩɩ wo.
42004014	Dɩ mɛ̃ Jeju bir na Thu Phuu fãga Galile, dɩ ɔɔ i kpaar dɩ khuirəəle fɛʋ.
42004015	Dɩ a-n dɩɩrɛ tɩbɩla awɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnana, dɩ wɛr fɛʋ n dʋbʋʋrɛ.
42004016	Dɩ Jeju jal Najarɛtɩ kãkɛ wɩ kɔɔ haanʋʋnɩ; dɩ hɩɩr wire a lʋʋn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra mɔ̃kɛra a-n kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ.
42004017	Dɩ mɔ̃ a ɩɩrnɩ a so sɛbɛ, Thãgbaa bobon Ejaɩɩ sɛbɛ wɩ haa. Dɩ a phubire sɛbɛra a yɩ kãkɛ gɩ kherenɩ ayɩ:
42004018	“Kɔ̃tɩnɩ Thu Phuu ha marɛ, gɩdonɩ a phiir mer ma-n mɩa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ bɔdarara. A thɔ̃ mɛr ma-n mιa deara wɩ 'lɛ taarɛ, na wɩrɛraakɛ na-n yɛna' dɩ wa yɩ. A thɔ̃ mɛr ɩ̃ taa wɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n kpooronɩ,
42004019	a na mɩana Kɔ̃tɩnɩ bɔ jɩ yɛ.”
42004020	Agɩpɩ dɩ khaan sɛbɛ a bir ha thɔ̃daar sa too. Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩle Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ bɩnɔɔle gaaraarɛ yire.
42004021	Dɩ a mar da-n mɩɩ wɩ: Nĩkɛ ga Thãgbaa sɛbɛ thɩmɩɩkɛ nɩ nɩɛnɩ daan pɩ.
42004022	Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n mɩιrɛ ɔɔda bɔ, dι dakha nʋɔ kpaa wɛr bɔ jɩ thɩmɩɩraakɛ n thɛnɩ ɔɔ nɔra, dɩ wa-n so: Ga do ɔr dʋɔn Jojɛfɩɩ bikuunaa?
42004023	Sɩ Jeju so warɛ: Gellakɛ na so marɛ sokpaakɛ anayɩ: Dɔtɔrɔ, kpɛɛnɛ afɩ khora dɩbara bɛɛ, gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ fɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ Kapɛrnayʋm dɩ sɩ nɩɛ, cʋɛ gɩ kɩɛr afɩ dʋɔ.
42004024	Dɩ a bire so war wo: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, wa-n bu Thãgbaa bobon bɩɛllakɛ ɔɔ dʋɔ bɔɔbɔa'.
42004025	Sobɔr mɩ so nar: Khikhɛra jɔɔjɔɔ kɔɔ hale Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩra Elɩɩ bɔɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ thãgba kɔɔ kurni yɛna yẽther na pora maadõ, dɩ kɔmɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ji dɩɩra fɛʋ.
42004026	Sɩ ɔbɔɔlerakɛ Thãgba na kɔɔ thɔ̃ ɔɔ bobon Elɩ khikhɛraraale bɩɛllakɛ, saagado khikhɛr bɩɛlɩkɛ hanɩ Sarɛpɩta Sɩdɔ̃ dɩɩraa pa gaaga.
42004027	Dɩ dakha gbulo bərəəm kɔɔ hale Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩra Thãgbaa bobon Elijee bɔɔ, sι bɩɛl wɛrrarakɛ na kɔɔ kpɛɛ, saagado Naamãakɛ dɔnɩ Siridaar gaaga.
42004028	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanι Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔɔle nɩɛnɩ gelela, nĩkhii fʋlɛ wɛr.
42004029	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ ɩɩr a tʋɔrʋʋ dɩ bɩnɔ thena, a jalna phaphapha a dana gɔ̃gɔ̃ horʋ wɩ dʋnaa ɓɛlɛnɔ, gɩdonɩ gɔ̃gɔ̃ yʋɔ awɩ dɩ ha.
42004030	Sɩ ɔr thɛthɛ dẽdẽdena a jal awɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn a thena.
42004031	Dɩ Jeju jaal Kapɛrnayʋm Galile dɩɩra, da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla hɩɩr wire.
42004032	Dɩ nʋɔ kpaa wɛr ɔɔ dɩɩrra gɩdonɩ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ hananɛ fãga.
42004033	Dɩ le kũu bɩɛl kɔɔ ha Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, kɛ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl, dɩ a hulene dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ:
42004034	Ee, anye sɩ ha kha na fɛr Najarɛtɩ Jeju? Fɩ ɩnɛ fɩ kʋɛ sɩ yaa? Mɩ jɩrɛ ntɛ fɩ donɩ: Thãgbaa Tɩɩ phu fι do.
42004035	Sɩ Jeju manaanɛ ayɩ: Pɩra, sa thɛ kuunnaale. Mɔ̃kɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuurə baanɩ thʋnɔ tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thιιn, a thιιraarɛ dιphã, sι aa cʋgʋʋ dιkharakɛ dιι puurə'.
42004036	Dι nʋɔ kpaa tιbιla fɛʋ dι wa-n mιι kha bιɛlbιɛl aa: Anyee thιmιι ca ha ʋrɛ? A-n mar kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔlasɔrarakɛ na fãga dι puno wi dι wa-n the.
42004037	Dι ɔɔ i kpaar dι khuirəəle fɛʋ.
42004038	Ɔbɔɔle Jeju thenι Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, a jaal a lõ Sιmɔ̃ɔ cɔ. Dι Sιmɔ̃ɔ khɛrι nι gι, a ji tomι kporre, dι wι phʋʋr Jeju dι wa-n pιɛ.
42004039	Dι Jeju pɔ gʋɛraa a phaan tomι kporre, dι tomι kporre ιιraa. Dι dapaara dι ιιr a tee wι kpakpaalɛ.
42004040	Wi lõ bɔɔ, wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hananι khodaraakɛ kho caar dιιdιι fʋnι, wι pɔna wɛr Jejura dι dɛ̃ɛ war fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl nyɛ̃ɛ, dι wι kpɛɛ.
42004041	Dι kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ dakha kɔɔ ther tιbιla bərəəmna, a hulẽ dι wa-n sona aa: Fɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun. Sι Jeju mana wɛr, aa-n tu wι mιa nʋɔa', gιdonι wι jιrɛ ɔr dʋɔn Kirisiti.
42004042	A dιι wιl Jeju ther jal khuirə, dι tibil jɔ mar dι wa-n ƴaalʋʋ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ wι yιιnι, wι-n yιrnaanɛ a na-n faa wa'.
42004043	Sι Jeju so warɛ: Gι teenanɛ ma-n mιι tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιιkɛ dɔnι Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda gɩ̃ dιsɔra dakha, gιdonι gɛrra Thãgba kɔɔ thɔ̃ mι.
42004044	Dι a hale Jude dιιra da-n mιι Thãgbaa thιmιι Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra.
42005001	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju hanι Jenejarɛtι mιιr nɔ nʋɔra, dι tibil jɔ kpa jιɛraa dι wa-n cɔ kha wι nιɛ Thãgbaa thιmιι,
42005002	a yɩrɛ mɩɩr nɔ nʋɔra gborõo yenyɔ, dɩ thʋ̃ phera gbuno wa-n cɔcɔɔ awɩ thʋ̃ pherdasɔ.
42005003	Dɩ a lʋʋn gborõ bɩɛllaakɛ dʋɔnnɩ Sɩmɔ̃ɔda, sa bɩɛlɛɛ ayɩ a tɔ gboroona, a hʋnɔnɛna thɩɩ gbe. Agɩpɩ dɩ too le gborõ bɩnɔ da-n dɩɩr tibil jɔ.
42005004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a dɩɩr wɩnɩ pɩ, a sor Sɩmɔna: Tɔ jala yɔ hulõ paar, nɩ dʋna anɩ thʋ̃ pherda gɩ fʋ thʋma.
42005005	Dɩ Sɩmɔ̃ birsee: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ kɔɔ dor thɔma na dɩtɩnɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka, sɩ sa kɔɔ fʋ thɩ̃a'. Sɩ gɩdonɩ fɛr sɔ, ma dʋnanɛ thʋ̃ pherdasɔra.
42005006	A wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ mɛ̃, wɩ 'lɛr thʋma tə̃tə̃tə̃, dɩ awɩ thʋ̃ pherdasɔ na-n kuur.
42005007	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ kher awɩ kuunsɔɔkɛ hanɩ gborõ kpɩɩra, wɩ pɔ a bulo ni. Dɩ wɩ pɔ a hi gborõo yenyɔɔle a tha thʋnɔ dɩ wa-n mʋʋ nyʋɔnɔ.
42005008	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Sɩmɔ̃ Pɩɛr yɩnɩ gele, a jire Jejuu ƴɛra sa sʋʋraa: Hʋnɔnɛna mɩ Kɔ̃tɩn, gɩdonɩ sopugodaar ha mɩ.
42005009	Gɩdonɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpagʋʋrɛ, ɔr nakha wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ hanaanɩ thʋmanaakɛ wɩ kɔɔ fʋnɩ.
42005010	Mɛ̃ gɩ kɔɔ ha dakha na Jakɩ, na Jã Jebedee bikuunsɔɔkɛ n buloni kha thɔma na Sɩmɔ̃. Sɩ dɩ Jeju so Sɩmɔna: Fa-n do maar n fʋ fa'. Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã tɩbɩla fa-n ƴaal mar thʋ̃ khaa.
42005011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ dananɩ gborõo thɩɩ, wɩ faarɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ sɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
42005012	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju kɔɔ hanɩ dɩ bɩɛlla, hɩnɛ kũu bɩɛl haleekɛ pala teenɩ tomɩr. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a yɩnɩ Jeju, a jire ɔɔ ƴɛra a sumo thɩɩra da-n phʋʋrʋʋ thakɛ ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado fɩ ture, fɩ punone cʋʋ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ gbuul pɩ.
42005013	Dɩ Jeju 'laa nyɔ̃ɔ a thaaraa sa so: Mɩ ture afɩ gbuul n pɛ. Dɩ dapaara gbuule pɩɩraa.
42005014	Agɩpɩ dɩ kpãkpaanaa a na-n so tibillə ga, sɩ a jala nɛna Thãgbaa bonɩ jidaar mɔ̃ a hanɩ, a 'laana phɔphʋɔl thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sonɩ, gɩ nɩna tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩ a kpɛɛrɛ.
42005015	Dι Jejuu i n kpaarɛ paar fɛʋ dɩ a-n pɛr, dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ bərəəm pʋɔraarɛ wɩ pɩɛ nũu, wɩ 'lɛna dakha kho kpɛɛrɛ.
42005016	Sɩ a sɩ warɛ sa the jal bəənnə a bɩɛl Thãgba.
42005017	Wi bɩɛl Jeju kɔɔ hale da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla. Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaraakɛ thɛnɩ Galile dɩɩra, na Jude dɩɩra, na Jerujalɛm dɩɩra fɛʋ, kɔɔ hale a too. Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ fãga n cʋʋrɛ Jeju da-n kpɛɛ khodara.
42005018	Dɩ hɩnɛ, tɩbɩla kɔɔ gbaar kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ gbãgbarnɛnɩ na jɔ̃ a pɔna, dɩ wa-n ƴaal wɩ lonaa wɩ pɛ Jejuu ƴɛra.
42005019	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ wa jɩnɩ ka wa lonaana', gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla jɔrɛ ka, wɩ jʋʋnaanɛ nãsʋrɔ a tona kaar na ɔɔ jɔ̃ Jejuu ƴɛra tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
42005020	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju yɩnɩ awι ha pɛ a sor: Ɩ̃ kuun, afɩ sopugosɔ hɛl farɛ.
42005021	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ mar dɩ wa-n so na awɩ bɩ̃ ayɩ: Amɛ ha ʋrɛ n kʋɛanɩ Thãgbaa i thakɛ? Amɛ n punone dɩ faa sopugosɔ saagado Thãgba gɩ dɩbara ga?
42005022	Dɩ Jeju jɩ mɔ̃ wɩ-n kpɩɛrnɩ awɩ bɩnɔ, a bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nɩ hana kpɩɛr caakɛ anɩ bɩnɔ?
42005023	Gɩmɔ̃ yɔɔnɛ sorra: Afɩ sopugosɔ hɛl farɛ gɩ yaa, agɩbo: Ɩrɛ a jala gɩ?
42005024	Sɩ mɔ̃ na fʋnɩ sɩ na jɩ, dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun hananɛ hʋɛ thɩɩra dɩ ɩ̃ faana sopugosɔ, mɩ so farɛ gbãgbarʋ, ιrɛ gba afɩ jɔ̃ na kɔna.
42005025	Dɩ dapaara dɩ ɩɩr awɩ ƴɛra a gba jɔ̃ɔkɛ a-n kɔɔ phɩnɔnɩ, a dʋbɩna Thãgbaa i da-n kɔna.
42005026	Dɩ nʋɔ kpaa tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩ wa-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i, dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ dɩ wa-n sona: Sɩ yɩrɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ nĩ waa.
42005027	A gele pɩ, Jeju ther a yɩ war gbadaar bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Levɩ, dɩ too war gba paar da-n tee war. Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Na kpa mar.
42005028	Dɩ Levɩ faa thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ sa ɩɩr da-n kpaaraa.
42005029	Dɩ Levɩ cʋʋraarɛ fɛtɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ɔɔ cɔ. Dɩ war gbadara jɔɔjɔɔ kɔɔ hale na wɩ̃ tibilsɔ dɩko kho paarra na wɛr.
42005030	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na-n hũhuun sa so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nɩ kho na-n yɔna na war gbadara nakha sopugodara?
42005031	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ga do tɩɩ khena n kɔɔ ƴaalɛ dɔtɔrɔa', sɩ wɩrɛ gɩ-n khonɩ gɩ.
42005032	Ga do fɩl sardara mɩ ɩ̃ ɩ̃ ƴaala', sɩ sopugodara wɛ dɩ wa debi haar.
42005033	Dɩ tɩbɩlaale sʋʋraa ayɩ: Jãa kpãkpãadara n lire nʋɔ tɔ̃tɔ̃tɔ̃ dɩ wa-n bɩɛlna Thãgba jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaraa kpãkpãadarasɔɔ kha, sɩ dɩ afɩ too wer n kho dɩ wa-n yɔna.
42005034	Dɩ Jeju so war: Na punone na cʋʋ wɩrɛ wɩ wenɩ herra dɩ wa li nʋɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ kha na khɛr he ya?
42005035	Sɩ wiresɔ na hale wa hɛl warnɩ khɛr he, dɩ dawisɔɔlera wa li nʋɔ dɩphã.
42005036	Dɩ a so warɛ sokpa bɩɛl wo: Tibil na ɓəər kẽkẽ phaa a bɛbɩna kẽkẽ tɩ̃a'. A a cʋʋ mɛ̃, ga dor a ɓəəre kẽkẽ phaale, sɩɩ do dakuruule a ɓəərni a bɛbɩna datɩ̃ɩ, ga ma kha ga.
42005037	Dɩ tibil na gba thʋʋrɩkɛ dɔnɩ daphaa na pɛr bʋla tɩɩna ga. A a cʋʋ mɛ̃, thʋ phaa na wɩɛlɛ bʋlaa sɩ na deer, gɩ do bʋlaale kʋɛrɛ mɛ̃.
42005038	Sɩ dɔ fɩ pɛ thʋ phaa bʋla phaara oti.
42005039	Tibilikɛ n dɛnɩ thʋ tɩ̃ɩ, a na ƴaal daphaa bã, gɩdonɩ a na sor nayɩ, thʋ tɩ̃ɩ n daanɔ.
42006001	Hɩɩr wi bɩɛl Jeju n kɔɔ kar a lõ jʋ lɩɛra. Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara 'laa a kha jɔ a fɔfɔrɔ a kho.
42006002	Dɩ wɩ̃ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n cʋʋ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ yɩnɩ gɩ-n sãsɩrɛ hɩɩr wire?
42006003	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Na kɔɔ yɩɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra gɩrɛɛkɛ Davɩdɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ kɔmɛr kɔɔ fʋʋnɩ ɔr na wɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ kha gaa?
42006004	Mee a kɔɔ lʋʋn Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ a gba buruukɛ wι-n hanι Thãgba a kho, sa ha wιrɛɛkɛ a hananι kha, sιrakɛ Thãgbaa gbõdara teana dιbara wι khɔ gι.
42006005	Sι dι so war: Mɛr tibili Bikuun dor Kɔ̃tιn hιιr wirerarakɛ.
42006006	Hιιr wi bιɛl wo, Jeju lʋʋn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, a ma da-n dιιr tιbιla. Dι le a yι kũu bιɛlιkɛ ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔ nyɔ̃ khini.
42006007	Dι jɔfʋ dιιrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara jʋʋr Jeju dι wa-n hιιn ado a na kpɛɛrɛ tibil khoo hιιr wire, gιdonι hʋɛ wι-n ƴaal wι pιɛraa sor.
42006008	Sι a jιrɛ mɔ̃ wι-n kpιɛrnι awι bιnɔ, a so kuunnaakɛ nyɔ̃ɔ khini ayι: Ɩrɛ jιlɛ kιɛr thɩ̃thιιn. Dι pal ιιr jιιl.
42006009	Dι Jeju so war: Mι-n bule ner, hιιr wire teana bɔ cʋʋrɛ yaa, puu cʋʋrɛ; agιbo fι taa tibil yaa, fι kʋʋ?
42006010	Sι a hιιn wɛr fɛʋ da-n finə sa bir so kuunnana: 'Laanɛ afι nyɔ̃; dι 'laa dιι do gι kpɛɛrɛ.
42006011	Dι nĩkhii fʋlɛ wι, dι wa-n gʋʋr kha awι ha mɔ̃ wa cʋʋnɩ Jejura.
42006012	Ɔbɔɔlera Jeju kɔɔ ther jal gɔ̃gʋɔna a bɩɛl Thãgba; dɩ a kɔɔ toore le a bɩɛl Thãgba dɩ dɩɩ wɩlna.
42006013	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩι wιlnι, a wer ɔɔ kpãkpãadara a phiir yʋɔr yenyɔ. Wɛr a ha ire thɔ̃thɔna:
42006014	Sιmɔ̃ ɔr a dʋ ire Pιɛr, sι ɔɔ õkuun n dɔ Ãdire, Jakι. Jã, Filipi, Bartelemι,
42006015	Matiə, Tomasι, Jakι Alfee bikuun,
42006016	na Sιmɔ̃ɔkɛ dʋɔnnι gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ tibil, Juudi Jakιι bikuun, na Judasιιkɛ thɛnι Karιyɔtι, kɛ kɔɔ debanι do lĩlir.
42006017	Dι Jeju gbũ nakha wɛr a jιιl gɔ̃gɔ̃ ɓɛlɛ̃ paar, kãkɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara jɔɔ hanι, na tibil jɔjʋɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃əkɛ thɛnι. Jude dιιra fɛʋ na Jerujalɛm, nakha Tιιr na Sιdɔ̃ dι khuirə kɛ hanι lanyɔ̃ nʋɔra.
42006018	Wι pɔr wι pɛ Jeju nũu wι 'lɛna kho kpɛɛrɛ. Dι wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbii n hʋɔlɔnι kɔɔ kpɛɛrɛ dakha.
42006019	Dι tibil jɔɔle fɛʋ n ƴaalɛ wa-n thaaraa, gιdonι fãga n thιιraarɛ dι a-n kpɛɛ wι fɛʋ.
42006020	Dι Jeju gba da-n hιιn ɔɔ kpãkpãadara sa so war ayι: Gι da nɛr bɔdarara, gιdonι Thãgbaa fãgadaar do dor anιda.
42006021	Gι da nɛrɛraakɛ kɔmɛr n fʋnι nɛnɛ̃, gιdonι na hire phi. Gι da nɛrɛraakɛ n khιanι, gιdonι na 'lɛr daʋ.
42006022	Gι da nar ɔbɔɔkɛ tιbιla na laar nιnι, ɔbɔɔkɛ wa lee nιnι na faa kpιι, wa-n nιιrna nι, wa-n kpɔrɔna nι ire dιι ho thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnι kpɔ̃kpɔrɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ tibili Bikuuni sora.
42006023	Na-n hana daʋ ga wiraalera a na kãkanɛ, gιdonι khaarda kɔ̃tɩ̃ι hale Thãgbaa dʋɔ dι a-n pιɛr nι. Gιdonι thalera awι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ cʋʋ Thãgbaa bobonasɔra.
42006024	Sι ga puu narɛ nɛrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnι lẽledara, gιdonι nι 'lɛr anι ha faa pι.
42006025	Ga puu narɛ nɛrɛɛkɛ n hienni, gιdonι kɔmɛr na fʋ nɛr. Ga puu narɛ nɛrɛɛkɛ n mananι nɛnɛ̃, gιdonι na har bιwɛra na yilẽbera.
42006026	Ga puu narɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ tιbιla fɛʋ n mιιnι anιda bɔ, gιdonι thale awι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ cʋʋ na wιrɛ kɔɔ dɔnι sõso bobonasɔ.
42006027	Sι mι so narɛ nɛrɛɛkɛ n pɛ mιnι nũu: Na-n na anι lãlaardara, na-n cʋɛ wιrɛ n laarɛ nιnι bɔɔ.
42006028	Na-n bɔna wιrɛɛkɛ n sɔna nιnι, na-n bιɛlnɛ Thãgba a na pɛ wιrɛraakɛ n hʋɔlɛ narnι.
42006029	A tibil ɓa fι gbʋa bιɛl, fe gbʋa kpιι a hanaa dakha. Dι a tibil gbaan afι darã, sιɛraa a gba afι kẽkẽ gburo dakha wo.
42006030	Tibil wo tibilikɛ n bιɛlnɛ farnι thɩ̃ɛ, hanaa, dι tibilikɛ gbaan fιnι thɩ̃ɛ, fa-n lʋʋra'.
42006031	Gιrɛɛkɛ nι-n ƴaalnι tιbιla na-n cʋɛ nar, na-n cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃ wɛrra dakha.
42006032	A na na wιrɛɛkɛ n naan nιnι, anye dɔ gιrɛ teronι a ha kpιι? Gιdonι sopugodara dakha wι-n nar wιrɛɛkɛ n naan wιnι.
42006033	Dι a na cʋʋ bɔɔ wɛkɛra n cʋɛ nɩnɩ bɔɔ, anye dɔ gɩrɛ teronɩ a ha kpɩɩ? Gɩdonɩ sopugodara dakha thalera wɩ-n cʋʋ.
42006034	Dɩ a wɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ-n pɛrnɩ haar wa yɩ gɛr na ha nɩ nɩ-n pemi thɩ̃ɛ, anye dɔ gɩrɛ teronɩ a ha kpɩɩ? Gɩdonɩ sopugodara dakha wɩ-n pemine kha awɩ ha, sɩ wa-n kpɩɛrna mɔ̃ wa birni na 'lɛ oti.
42006035	Sɩ na-n na anɩ lãlaardara, na-n cʋɛ bɔɔ, na-n pema tɩbɩla sɩ na-n kpɩɛr nɩ birə 'lɛrɔ dɩkha ga. Dɩ mɛ̃ na 'lɛ khaarda kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, dɩ na dor dakha Kəkəədaarɩ bɩsãsɔ, gɩdonι a bɔrɛ tɩɩ kʋɛara na tɩɩ puusɔra.
42006036	Gɛr gɩ nɩ dɔ bɔ jɩ tɩbɩla, mɔ̃ anɩ Thɩ donɩ bɔ jɩdaar.
42006037	Na-n fi do kɩɩldara ga, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba na do nar Kɩɩldaara'. Na-n heen tibil sora', dɩ mɛ̃ na 'lɛ so heene dakha ga. Na-n faa tɩbɩlaa dɩ pa a na hana wɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba na faa anɩ dɩ pa a na ha nɩ dakha.
42006038	Na-n 'laanɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba na 'laa a na ha nɩ dakha. Ga dor mɩɛda bʋɔɔkɛ wa ɩɩnɩ a na yɛyɛɛ gɩ hi ga-n jal wɩ ha nɩ. Gɩdonɩ mɩɛda ca ʋrɛɛkɛ nɩ-n kɔɔ mɩɛnanɩ thɩ̃ɛ, ɔrra Thãgba na mɩɛna a na ha nɩ oti.
42006039	Dɩ Jeju so warɛ sokpaa wo ayɩ: Yaarʋ na punone na thɔɔ yaarʋ ya? Mee wɛr yenyɔ fɛʋ na jiire kõkorro.
42006040	Kpãkpãadaar na hale a na kɔ̃tɩ̃ na jɔ ʋrɛ n dιrɛɛna', sι ɔbɔɔkɛ a na dιιrnι na pι, a na har mɔ̃kɛ ʋrɛ dιrɛɛnι hanι.
42006041	Mɔ̃gιdo dι fι ka gar yire hɔ̃ phɩɩnaakɛ hanɩ afɩ omii yiro, sɩ fa-n ka dɩ fɩ hɩɩn kparrɛɛkɛ hanɩ afɩ thɛthɛɛ yiroə?
42006042	Dɩ mɔ̃ fa fʋ sɩ na so afɩ omina nayɩ: Ɩ̃ omi, jɩlɛ ɩ̃ ti hɔ̃ phɩ̃ɩkɛ ha fɩnɩ yiro, fɛrɛɛkɛ na yɛnɩ kparrɛɛkɛ hanɩ afɩ yiroə? Fɛr bɩnɛ yenyɔdaar, te kparrɛɛkɛ hanɩ afɩ yiro ɓo, le fa jɩɩ yɩ hɔ̃ phɩ̃ɩkɛ hanɩ afɩ omii yiro a na ti.
42006043	Thɩr bʋɔ na puno na se bi puə'. Dɩ thɩrʋʋkɛ na bʋɔnɔna' na puno na se bi bʋɔ dakha ga.
42006044	Gɩdonɩ be wɩ-n jɩna thɩra fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl. Sobɔr gɩ, wa-n yɛɛ bara usɩɛra ga, dɩ wa-n khʋ̃ ɓãɓar be paabɩrʋra dakha ga.
42006045	Tɩɩ bʋɔ n tire dabʋɔɔkɛ hanɩ ɔɔ hara dɩ thena, sɩ tɩɩ puu n tire dapuukɛ hanɩ ɔɔ hara dɩ thena. Gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ n henɩ haarra, gɛr n thɛ nɔɔ.
42006046	Mɔ̃gιdo dι na-n we mι Kɔ̃tιn, Kɔ̃tιn, sι na-n cʋʋ gιrɛ mι-n so narna'.
42006047	Tibil wo tibilikɛ ιna marnι da-n nιɛ ɩ̃ thιmɩɩ dɩ gbuuro yʋʋ da-n cʋʋ, ma nι narɛ ntɛɛkɛ a honι.
42006048	A hʋrɛ tibilikɛ n mɛnɩ cʋɔr, a kpe koru dιι hulono dɩ kpɛɛrɔ go kʋʋ boka nã thɛrɛɛra. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nyʋɔn phanɩ, dɩ poo be dɩ a-n cɩr cʋɔrɩle, sɩ ga puno cʋʋ thɩ̃a', gɩdonɩ kuunile mɩɩrɛ dɩɩ bɔr.
42006049	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n nɩɛnɛnɩ sɩ aa-n cʋa', a hʋrɛ tibilikɛ thɛnɩ cʋɔr thɩ bʋraara, sɩ aa kpe koru a kpɛɛrɔ go kʋa'. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ poo benɩ dɩ a-n cɩr cʋɔrɩle, dɩɩ do dapaara gɩ derre, dɩ cʋɔrɩle jire ji puure.
42007001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩsɔɔkɛ fɛʋ tɩbɩlalaakɛ n pɩɛnɩ nũu dɩɩ pɩ, a jaal Kapɛrnayʋm.
42007002	Dɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hale dɩ ga-n kho ɔɔ thɔ̃daar bɩɛlɩkɛ a-n nanɩ dɩɩ ka, dɩ dã khir.
42007003	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle nɩɛnɩ Jejuuda, a thʋɔnaanɛ wɩ̃ Juifi kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, wɩ jala a bɩɛlnɛɛ a pɔ a kpɛɛnɛ ɩnɩ thɔ̃daar.
42007004	Dɩ wɩ pɔ dã Jeju a phʋʋrʋʋ dɩ wa-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛna thakɛ ayɩ: Kuunikɛ teenanɛ fɩ cʋʋraa gele.
42007005	Gɩdonɩ a-n nar asɩ ca, dɩ ɔr gɩɩkɛ kɔɔ mɛnɩ asɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ.
42007006	Dɩ Jeju jal nakha wɛr. Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ a-n wɔrɔnɩ cʋɔr, sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle thʋɔn ɔɔ kuunsɔ wɩ sʋɔraa ayɛ: Kɔ̃tɩn, fa-n thʋ̃ vɔɔ mã', gɩdonɩ ma teena dɩ fa lõ ɩ̃ cɔa'.
42007007	Gelela dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma kɔɔ teena ɩ̃ pɔ dɩbara afɩ pa ga; sɩ sɔ thɩmɩɩ bi bɩɛl dɩbara, ɩ̃ thɔ̃daar na kpɛɛrɛ.
42007008	Gɩdonɩ mɛrɛɛkɛ, mɩ hananɛ ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔkɛ jɔ mɩnɩ, dɩ mɩ hananɛ dakha sɔrasɛsɔɔkɛ mɩ jɔnɩ. A mɩ so bɩɛlla: Jala, dɩ jal. A mɩ so bɩɛlla wo ayɩ, a ɩna, dɩ ɩ̃. A mɩ so ɩ̃ thɔ̃daarra: Cʋɛ gɩrɛ, dɩ cʋʋ.
42007009	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ ga thɩmɩɩle, nʋɔ kɔɔ kpagʋʋrɛ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩdaraale. Dɩ Jeju kɩɩl a so tibil jɔraale n kpaaraanɩ ayɩ: Mɩ so narɛ Ɩjɩrayɛl dɩɩrarakɛ ma kɔɔ yɩ tibil dɩ hana ha pɛrɛ thaka'.
42007010	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ thɔ̃thɔnaale kɔɔ kɛrnɩ na bir cʋɔrɔ, wɩ yɩrɛ thɔ̃daarɩle dɩ hana tomɩ kheu.
42007011	Agɩpɩ Jeju jaal dɩ bɩɛllaakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Naɩn, dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara na tibil jɔ kɔɔ cʋrrɛ kha dɩ wa-n jal.
42007012	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n wɔrɔnɩ dɩ lõfonʋɔ, hɩnɛ wɩ gbaar khire dɩ wa-n jalna dʋ paar. Khikhɛr bɩɛlɩ bi bɩɛlla gɩ 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ dɩ hana, dɩ dɩdara jɔɔ kɔɔ har kha na khikhɛrʋʋle.
42007013	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Kɔ̃tιn yιιnι, bʋɔ fʋʋrɛ dι sʋʋraa: Fa-n khιa'.
42007014	Agιpι dι tɔ pɔ a thar khi gbadaara. Dι wιrɛ gbaannι khire jιιl. Dι Jeju so khireraale ayι: Daɓolbir mι so farɛ, ιrɛ.
42007015	Dι khire pal ιιr a too a ma da-n mιι thιmιa. Dι Jeju kpaa a ha ɔɔ nι.
42007016	Dι maar fʋlɛ tιbιla fɛʋ, dι wa-n dʋbι Thãgbaa i dι wa-n sona: Thãgbaa bobon kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιɛl ιrɛ asι thɩ̃thιιn. Dι Thãgba ιnɛ dakha a kher ɔɔ too.
42007017	Dι thιmιιrιle cʋʋrɛ Jejuuda dιι kpaar paar fɛʋ Judera na dι khuirə fɛʋ.
42007018	Jã kɔɔ nιɛrɛ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔlera fɛʋ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara mιgʋʋnι, dι a wer ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara yenyɔ,
42007019	a thɔ̃ wι Kɔ̃tιnna wι bulenee ayɛ: Fɛr dʋɔn ʋrɛɛkɛ na ιnanι yaa, agιbo dɔ sa-n pιɛr tιι kpιι?
42007020	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ tιbιlaale danι Jejuu pa, wι sʋʋraarɛ: Jã Batιsιtι thɔna sι sι bulene fi ayɛ: Fɛr dʋɔn ʋrɛɛkɛ na ιnanι yaa, agιbo dɔ sa-n pιɛr tιι kpιι?
