42007021	Ga bɔraalera Jeju kpɛɛrɛ khodara jɔɔ na wιrɛɛkɛ hananι taansɔ, a weena dakha kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔla, a khɛrna yarasɔ jɔɔjɔɔ yinə.
42007022	Dι Jeju birse wi: Nι kɛra birə a sɔ Janana gιrɛɛkɛ nι yιnι, na gιrɛɛkɛ nι nιɛnι: Yarasɔ n yιrɛ, nɛ kʋɛdara n sar bɔɔbɔɔ, gbulosɔɔ gbuul pιrɛ, dι nʋrasɔ khɛrrɛ, dι khesɔ n ιιrɛ dι wι the khirera, dι bɔdara nιɛrɛ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι.
42007023	Sι gι da ʋrɛraakɛ ma doronι nɛ baradaa ga.
42007024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wιrɛ Jã thɔnι kɔnι pι, Jeju mar da-n mιι tibil jɔɔle Jãadara: Anye nι kɔɔ jal a hιιn bəənnə? Poo balãsιιkɛ n khəəfəneni gι ya?
42007025	Dι anye nι kɔɔ jal yι? Kuunikɛ n tɔnι kẽkẽ ɓʋ̃ɔ gι ya? Nι hιnɛ wιrɛɛkɛ n tʋɔnnι kẽkẽ ɓɔna dι wa-n khona dιko bʋɔ, fãgadaraa cɔ wι-n ha.
42007026	Dι anye nι kɔɔ jal yι? Thãgbaa bobon gι ya? Mι so narɛ, sobɔr gι, bιɛlιkɛ jɔnι Thãgbaa bobon gι.
42007027	Jã dʋɔn ʋrɛɛkɛ wι kɔɔ khereronι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Hιnɛ, mɛr Thãgba thɔna ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃, dι na kʋʋl fι ƴιɛ, a gbɛbιrι fι hʋɛ afι ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ.”
42007028	Dι mι so narɛ, wιrɛ fɛʋraakɛ khɛra n kɔnιι thɩ̃thιιn, bιɛl na hale a kɔ̃tɩ̃ jɔ Jã ga. Dι ʋrɛ kanι do dabuu fιιʋ Thãgba fãgadaarι dιra, a kɔ̃tιnɛ a jɔ Jã.
42007029	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tιbιla fɛʋ na war gbadara nιɛnι Jãa nɔ, wι jιrɛ dι Thãgba sarrɛ, a tu dι Jã kɔɔ kpɛɛ wι nyʋɔnɔ.
42007030	Sι jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ wer kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaal warnɩ dɩɩ debi a do mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ wɛrra, mɔ̃kɛ wɩ bonɩ Jãa yɔ kpɛɛ.
42007031	Ana ma cʋna nĩdaraakɛ dɩphã, dɩ ana wɩ hona ya fɛ?
42007032	Wɩ hʋrɛ bɩsanasɔɔkɛ n tɔɔnɩ ƴatɔɔ, dɩ wa-n we kha bɩɛlbɩɛl dɩ wa-n so: Sɩ kɔɔ ʋnɛ bɩɩl nɛrɛra, sɩ na kɔɔ sa ga. Sɩ kɔɔ khɩɩrɛ nɛrɛra, sɩ na kɔɔ dea'.
42007033	Gɩdonɩ Jã Batɩsɩtɩ kɔɔ ɩnɛ, aa-n kho dɩkora', aa-n yɔ taan dakha ga, dɩ nɩ so: Kɔ̃tɛɛbuu hanaanɛ.
42007034	Dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ɩ̃ wo, a thɩ̃ɛ mɩ-n kho, a thɩ̃ɛ mɩ-n yɔ dɩ nɩ so: Hɩnɛ, kũu kɛ̃kɛbɩ gɩ a dona ta yɔn, war gbadara na sopugodaraa kuun gɩ.
42007035	Sɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n tuonni Thãgbaa kpɛsɛ n nɩnanɛ dɩ sobɔr har kpɛsɛrɛɛlee pa.
42007036	Jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar bɩɛl gɩ, a we Jeju a pɔ ɩnɩ-n kho kha dɩkor. Dɩ Jeju lõ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaarɩlee cɔra, a too dɩko kho paar.
42007037	Dɩ hɩnɛ, khɛ sopugodaar bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hale dɩ bɩnɔ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a nɩɛnɩ dɩ Jeju hale jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaarɩ cɔ da-n kho dɩkor, a pɔnanɛ latɩkolo na laaso ja bʋlabir;
42007038	a gulẽgana Jejuu nɛ khʋra da-n khɩɩna, sa ma da-n huro Jejuu nɛ na yilẽbe. Agɩpɩ dɩ pɩɩn na ɔɔ yʋsũ sa pal Jejura nɛɛ, da-n thir latιkolola.
42007039	Ɔbɔɔkɛ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaarιle kɔɔ wɛnι Jeju yιɛnι, a sor ɔɔbara ayι: Ado Thãgbaa bobon kuunikɛ do, a na jιrɛ khɛrιkɛ n thaaraanι, ntɛ a donι na mɔ̃kɛ a hanɩ: Khɛr sopugodaar gɩ.
42007040	Dɩ Jeju so: Sɩmɔ̃, mɩ hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ a na so far. Dɩ birsee: Dɩɩrdaar, mɩa.
42007041	Dɩ Jeju so: Tibil bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n kɔɔ peminoni war kɔɔ hale, dɩ tɩbɩla hanaa helu. Cacadaarɩda daan wire taamɔɩ thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ war; sɩ balanyɔdaarɩda dã wire kpalanyɔ yʋɔr thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ war.
42007042	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ wa-n yɩɛnɩ a na lɩmʋa', a faarɛ a ha wɩ fɛʋ yenyɔra. Ʋmɔ̃ wɛr yenyɔraale na naanɛɛ a na jɔ?
42007043	Dɩ Sɩmɔ̃ birsee: Mɩ pɛrɛ haar ʋrɛɛkɛɛ hel jʋɔnɔnɩ gɩ. Dɩ Jeju birsee: Sobɔr fɩ so.
42007044	Agɩpɩ dɩ kɩɩl da-n hɩɩn khɛrɩle sa bule Sɩmɔ̃: Fɩ yɩrɛ khɛrɩkɛɛ? Afɩ cɔ mɩ lõ sɩ fa kɔɔ ha mɩ nyʋɔn ɩ̃ cɔcɔɔnɛ nɛa', sɩ khɛrɩkɛ hurone mi nɛɛ na ɔɔ yilẽbi sa bir a pɩɩnna ɔɔ yʋsũ.
42007045	Fa kɔɔ pal mɩ a fʋɔr ma', sɩ khɛrɩkɛ a fʋna bɔɔkɛ mι lonι a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ, aa sιrɔrakɛ kpιι ɩ̃ nɛ pala'.
42007046	Fa kɔɔ bʋl mι niin yʋʋra ga, sɩ khɛrɩkɛ a kɔɔ bʋl mɛr latιkolo nɛɛ.
42007047	Gɛr gι mι so farɛ, Thãgba faarɛ ɔɔ sopugookɛ kɔɔ jʋɔnɔnιnakɛ a haa, gιdonι khɛrιkɛɛ naʋ jɔrɛ; dι ʋrɛɛkɛ Thãgba faanι sopugo gbe a ha, gbera ɔɔ naʋ n ha dakha.
42007048	Dι Jeju so khɛrraale: Thãgba faarɛ afι sopugosɔ a ha fι.
42007049	Dι wιrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ hananι kha dιko kho paar mar dι wa-n so awιbarara aa: Amɛ ha ʋrɛ dι ba faarakɛ sopugosɔ ya fɛ?
42007050	Sι Jeju so khɛrraale: Afι ha pɛ taa fι, kɔna na ha ɩɩ.
42008001	Agɩpɩ Jeju kɔɔ jaal da-n kpaar dɩ kɔ̃tɩnana na dɩ biisɔra, da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla da-n mɩɩna tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda.
42008002	Dɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ kɔɔ har kha na ɔr, na wɩ̃ khɛrsɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ weeronɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔlasɔ a faa a kpɛɛna khoosɔ. Marɩɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Magɩdala, kɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbii makonyɔ kɔɔ thɩɩrɔnɩ gɩ,
42008003	na Janɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Kuja, Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ thɔ̃daraa hɩɩndaarɩ khɛr, na Sujan, na wɩ̃ khɛrsɔ bərəəmkɛ n kɔɔ buloni Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara na awɩ thɩ̃sɔ.
42008004	Tɩbɩlaakɛ thɛnɩ dɩɩsɔra fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl pɔr Jejura. Mɔ̃ tibil jɔjʋɔɔle kpanɩ kha a jɛ, a so warɛ sokpaakɛ ayɩ:
42008005	Bi jaldaar gɩ, a the da-n jal be. Dɩ mɔna a-n jalnɩ yɛ̃ bi jire hʋɛra, dɩ tɩbɩla saar na nɛɛ, dɩ 'lominə pɔ uul.
42008006	Yɛ̃ bi ji gbãgbã nã thɛrɛɛra. Ɔbɔɔkɛ gɩ phuni pɩ, gɩ khire gɩdonɩ ga-n yɩ thɩ mɩ̃a'.
42008007	Yɛ ji wo uu thɩ̃thɩɩn a gbɛbɩna uusɔ, a phu dɩ uu sɩlã gɩ.
42008008	Yɛ ji thɩ bʋɔra. Ɔbɔɔkɛ gɩ phuni pɩ, gɩ ɩnɛ a bɩ̃ dɩ a-n kakɛ tamaa. Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju sonɩ thale pɩ, a hulene ayɩ: Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
42008009	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara bulee sokpaalee kɩrra.
42008010	Dɩ birse wi ayɩ: Nɛr Thãgba kɔɔ ha nɩ jɛ thɩ̃ gbulikɛ dʋɔnnɩ ɔɔ fãgadaar doda. Sɩ ʋkhasɔ sokpaa wɩ-n sona war, dɩ mɛ̃ “wa-n hɩɩn sɩ wa yɩ ga, wa-n nɩɛ dakha sɩ wa jɩ kɩrʋa'.”
42008011	Sokpaakɛɛ kιrra ha gιrɛ: Thãgbaa so dʋɔn be.
42008012	Wιrɛ hɔnι hʋ nʋɔ wɛr dɔ wιrɛ na-n nιɛnɛnι, agιpι Satã n pɔ dι ti sorιle awι hara, gι do nɔɔ wa pɛr haar wι 'lɛna dakha taara'.
42008013	Wιrɛ hɔnι gbãgbã nã thɛrɛɛ wɛr dɔ wιrɛ na-n nιɛnɛnι Thãgbaa so, dι wι tu na daʋ, sι wa-n sιrɔ Thãgbaa so dιι yι nɛ gɔ paara', dιι do bɔɔ gbe wι pɛr haar dιbara. Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ fifiləle n dã wιnι, wι-n kɛrnanɛ khiru.
42008014	Sι gιrɛɛkɛ jenι u ballɔ hʋɔn wιrɛɛkɛ n nιɛnɛnι Thãgbaa so, sι mɔ̃ wι-n ιιrnι hʋɛrara, dɛr na ler, na gιrɛ n danι tibil haar n sιlã wɛr, dι wa-n se beekɛ leana'.
42008015	Sι gιrɛ jenι thι bʋɔra hʋɔn wιrɛɛkɛ na-n nιɛnɛnι Thãgbaa so dι wι fʋ gι na bɩ̃ bʋɔ, na fιl telẽe a na se be na yιrrɛ.
42008016	Tibil na pɛr dɔɔ lãphana sι agιpι a gba a suuro bιlãkpʋʋnna, agιbo a to kakala ballɔa', sι bilela a na dɛ̃ɛ wιrɛ n lonanι n yι dahιrɛ.
42008017	Gιdonι thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ker sι ga do wι cʋʋrɛ dιι thaa ga, dι thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ha gbul sιι do wa jι gaaga, gι do dakha wo ga yιraa ga.
42008018	Na-n jιɛ dʋ bʋrɛ mɔ̃kɛ nι-n nιɛnι, gιdonι ʋrɛɛkɛ hananι thɩ̃ɛ, Thãgba na bire na haa na dɛbιrɔ; sι ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananι thɩ̃a', Thãgba na tiirəərerakɛ phubi gιrɛɛkɛ a-n kpιɛrnι ιnι hananɛ.
42008019	Dι Jejuu õkũu bιnɔsɔ na ɔɔ nι kɔɔ pʋɔraarɛ, sι wa puno a na dãa ga gιdonι tιbιla jɔrɛ.
42008020	Dι wι sʋʋraa aa: Afɩ nɩ na afɩ õkũu bɩnɔsɔ hale phiilo dɩ wa-n ƴaal wɩ yɩ fɩ.
42008021	Dɩ birse wi: Ɩ̃̃̃ nɩ na ɩ̃ õkona dɔ wɩrɛɛkɛ n pɛnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ nũu, dɩ wɩ yɩr dɩ wa-n cʋʋ.
42008022	Wi bɩɛl Jeju kɔɔ lʋʋn gboroona na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, sa so war ayɩ: Nɩ dɔ sɩ iir iiro; dɩ wɩ jaal.
42008023	Mɔ̃kɛ wɩ hanɩ phɛllɔ Jeju daarɛ. Dɩ dapaara jɛkhure ɩɩrɛ na fãga mɩɩr nɔɔra, dɩ nyʋɔn ma dɩ ga-n hi gborõo, dι thɩ̃ɛ na-n bɔ war bã.
42008024	Dι wι tɔ dã a jaa Jeju a sʋʋraa: Dιιrdaar, dɩɩrdaar, sι-n buure. Dι mɛ̃ a jaa a mana jιɛ na nyʋɔnιkɛ n uboni dιι pιr, dι thɩ̃ɛ na-n tutugo bã.
42008025	Sι agιpι dι bule wi: Kana anι ha pɛ ha? Sι maar kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr dι nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wι, dι wa-n bule khasɔ bιɛlbιɛl aa: Anyee tibil ca ha ʋrɛ, dι punonakɛ jιɛ na mιιr nɔ nyʋɔnnakɛ dι ga-n nιι nũu?
42008026	Dɩ wι kɔɔ daan dιιkɛ dɔnι Jerajedaraa dʋɔ, kɛ hanι ka Galile dιι pɛnι ƴιɛ.
42008027	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju gbuni thιιra, dʋɔdaar bιɛlιkɛ hananι kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ caanʋʋnɛ. Gι kɔɔ maanɛ kɛkɛkɛ aa-n kɔɔ tonι kɩ̃kιɩna', aa-n cɔ cʋɔrɔa', sι khi dʋ paarsɔ a-n cɔ.
42008028	Mɔna a yɩnɩ Jeju, a hulene a jinə ɔɔ ƴɛra sa phã nɔ khɩɩr ayɩ: Anye mɩ ha kha na fɛr Jeju, Thãgba Kəkəədaarɩ Bikuun? Mɩ-n phʋʋr fɛr fa-n hʋɔl mara'.
42008029	Gɩdonɩ Jeju kɔɔ sʋʋraarɛ: A fɩ jɩ thɛ. Kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔlɩle kɔɔ mãa hana kuunikɛ kɛkɛkɛ, dɩ wɩ linəə jɔrkɔ a baranaa nɛɛ na ther a na bɛr, sɩrakɛ a-n khaarɛ lidaale sɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbuule n halʋʋ dɩ jalna bəənnəsɔ.
42008030	Dι Jeju bulee: Mɔ̃ afι i n do? Dι birsee: Dajɔ gι. Gιdonι kɔ̃tɛɛbi jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ lonanaa.
42008031	Dι wι-n phʋʋrɛ Jeju a na-n wee nι a faa kõkorʋra ga.
42008032	Sι dabulo sιthɔsɔ kɔɔ hale jɔɔ gɔ̃gʋɔna dι wa-n khʋʋl. Dι kɔ̃tɛɛbiirə phʋʋr Jeju a ha nɩ hʋɛ ɩnɩ-n lõ sɩthɔsɔraale bɩnɔ, dɩ ha wɩ hʋɛ.
42008033	Dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ thɩɩr kuunnaale a jal a lõ sɩthɔsɔraale bɩnɔ a tinə wi le gɔ̃gɔ̃ horo, dɩ wɩ caalɛ a jiir mɩɩr nɔɔra a khiir.
42008034	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩrɛ n khɛ wɩnɩ yɩnɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ dananɩ, wɩ kɔɔ car kɔ̃ a mɩɩ dɩɩra na kõgosora mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛle hanɩ.
42008035	Dɩ tɩbɩla the jal hɩɩn gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananɩ; dɩ wɩ pɔr Jejura, a yɩ kuunile kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ kɔɔ thɩɩrɔnɩ dɩ too Jejuu kal ƴɔɔ, a to kɩ̃kɩɩn a hanana dakha yʋ bʋɔ. Dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ fɛʋ.
42008036	Dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ yɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛɛle cʋɛnɩ mɩɩ wɛr mɔ̃kɛ Jeju taanɩ kuunile kɔɔ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbii.
42008037	Dɩ Jerajedara fɛʋ kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ Jeju a thɛ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa faa wɩ, gɩdonɩ maar kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr dɩɩ ka.
42008038	Dɩ Jeju lõ gborõo a bir da-n kɔ̃. Dɩ kuunilera kɔ̃tɛɛbii kɔɔ thɩɩrɔnɩ phʋʋrʋʋ a dɔ ɩnɩ-n do ɔɔ totoo. Sɩ Jeju bor sa sʋʋraa:
42008039	Birə kɔna afɩ cɔ a mɩa thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ cʋʋ farnɩ. Dɩ mɛ̃ a jal a mɩɩ paar fɛʋ dɩɩraale gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Jeju kɔɔ cʋʋraanɩ.
42008040	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ kɛrnɩ bir, tɩbɩla fɛʋ teguure, gɩdonɩ wɩ-n kɔɔ pɩɛrʋʋrɛ fɛʋ.
42008041	Sɩ hɩnɛ, kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jaɩrʋsɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tιn Juifisɔɔ Thagba fʋɔr cɔra pɔr, a ji Jejuu ƴɛ thɩ̃thιɩn da-n phʋʋrʋʋ a pɔ ιnι cɔ.
42008042	Gιdonι a hananɛ khebi bιɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ dι thɔɔ yɛna yʋɔr yenyɔ, kɛ n khenι. Dι mɔ̃ Jeju hanι jaal, tibil jɔɔle thʋnɛ gbʋɔrʋʋ ka.
42008043	Dι khɛ bιɛl gι, a hale a hana tɩ̃ι a cʋʋna yɛna yʋɔr yenyɔ, dι a kɔɔ kʋɛrɛ thιdarara ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ a hananι fɛʋ, sι tibil bιɛllakɛ na kɔɔ puno a kpɛsɛa'.
42008044	Dι a tɔr pɔ Jejuu khiro a thaaraa kẽkẽ nʋɔra; dι dapaara ɔɔ tɔmɩ̃ theele kur.
42008045	Dι Jeju bule aa: Amɛ thaan mar? Mɔ̃kɛ tιbιla fɛʋ n bananι Pιɛr sʋʋraarɛ: Dιιrdaar, tibil jɔ wer hi far thaa dι wa-n cʋɔr fι, sι dι fa-n bule amɛ thaan farι?
42008046	Dι Jeju birse: Tibil tha marɛ, gιdonι mι jιrɛ fãga kɔɔ the marɛ gbe.
42008047	Ɔbɔɔkɛ khɛrιlera yιɛnι dιι do Jeju jιnaanɛ, a pɔr na jẽu a ji Jejuu ƴɛra, a so tιbιla fɛʋʋ ƴɛ thɩ̃thιιn mɔ̃ dɔnι kιrʋ dι ιnι kɔɔ thaaraa na mɔ̃kɛ ιnι kɔɔ kpɛɛnι dapaara khə̃khə̃.
42008048	Dι Jeju sʋʋraa: Ɩ̃ bikhɛr, afι ha pɛ taa fι, kɔna na ha ιι.
42008049	Mɔ̃ a hanι mιιrɔ, tibil bιɛl ther Jaιrʋsι kɔ̃tιnι cɔ, a pɔ so Jaιrʋsιra aa: Afι bikhɛr khire. Fa-n vɔɔ Dιιrdaar bã.
42008050	Sι mɔ̃ Jeju kɔɔ nιɛnι gele, a sor Jaιrʋsιra: Fa-n do haar n ubi fa', sι pιɛr haar dιbara dι a na ler.
42008051	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ danι cʋɔr aa tu tibil n lona kha na ɔr, saagado Pιɛr na Jakι na bιsaanιlee thι na ɔɔ nι gaaga.
42008052	Tιbιla fɛʋ n khιιrɛ dι wa-n bιna. Dι Jeju so: Na-n khιa' aa khə', sι a-n daarɛ.
42008053	Sι wι-n maanʋʋnɛ gɩdonɩ wɩ jɩrɛ a khire.
42008054	Sɩ dɩ fʋʋ nƴɔ̃ɔ sa so nɔ khɩɩr: Bɩsaan, pala ɩrɛ.
42008055	Dɩ ɔɔ fesu kɛr birəə, dɩ pal dapaara a ɩɩr. Dɩ Jeju so war aa, dɔ wɩ haa dɩkor a kho.
42008056	Dɩ nʋɔ kpaa khebiri thɩ na nɩrɛ, sɩ Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ wa-n so tibillə gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ danana'.
42009001	Dɩ Jeju wer yʋɔr yenyɔ a ha wɩ fãga na punone kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔra fɛʋ, wa-n kpɛɛna khodara dakha.
42009002	A thɔ̃ wɛr wɩ jala a na mɩa Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda a na kpɛɛna khodara.
42009003	Sɩ a so warɛ: Na-n gba thɩ̃ɛ fʋrɔ jalna kpaar paar, dɩ gbʋʋl gɩ, dɩ kpakpaar lokaar gɩ, dɩ buru gɩ, dɩ war ga. Na-n fʋrɔ dakha kẽkena yenyɔa'.
42009004	Dɩ cʋɔr wo cʋɔrɩkɛ na lonɩ, nɩ tɔɔ le a kɔnana.
42009005	Sɩ ado pa dɔɔkɛ wa tee nɩna', a na the le dɩ dɔɔraale, nɩ kpɛɛnɛ thɩlãkobeekɛ ma nιnι nɛɛ a faa war gι nιna wι thιmιιr.
42009006	Dɩ kpãkpãadara jaal dɩ wa-n kpaar dɩɩra dɩɩra, dɩ wa-n mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, dɩ wa-n kpɛɛna khodara paar fɛʋ.
42009007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar buu kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ fɛʋ n cʋɛnɩ, ɔɔ kpɩɛr nyanyaanɛ fɛʋ, gɩdonɩ wɩ̃ tibil n sor ayɩ: Jã Batɩsɩtɩ gɩ, ɔr ɩrɛ the khirera.
42009008	Ɩkhasɔ n yɩ wo: Elɩ gɩ, a nɩna ɔɔbara. Wɛ n yɩ: Mama Thãgbaa bobon bɩɛl ɩrɛ a the khirera.
42009009	Dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ sor: Mee mɩ kɔɔ kʋrɛ Jã a kur yʋʋ, sɩ amɛ ha ʋrɛ mɩ-n nɩɛrɔnɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ? Dɩ mɛ̃ a ƴaal ɩnɩ-n yɩɩ.
42009010	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ thɔ̃thɔna kɛrnɩ bir, wɩ mɩɩrɛ Jeju gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnι. Dι kpa wι kana pa kpιι Bɛcaιda dι khʋra.
42009011	Sι ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil jɔɔle nιɛnι wι kpaanɛ. Dι Jeju tee wer a mιι wι Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda, a kpɛɛna dakha wιrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnι kho kpɛɛrɛ.
42009012	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ dιι n dʋɔrnι, yʋɔr yenyɔɔle pɔr a sʋʋraa aa: Bɩlanɛ tibil jɔɔkɛ wι jal dι biisɔra na kõgosoraakɛ wɔrɔnɛnι, wɩ cɔ wɩ ƴaalna dakha dɩkɔ wɩ kho, gɩdonɩ kɩɛrɩkɛ sɩ hanɩ bəənnə gɩ.
42009013	Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n hana wɩ dɩkɔ wɩ kho; sɩ dɩ wɩ birsee: Buru yemɔɩ dɩbara sɩ hana na thʋma yenyɔ, agado sɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ jala a the dɩkɔ a ha tɩbɩla fɛʋʋka'.
42009014	Sɩ tɩbɩlaale kɔɔ thɔɔrɛ gbɩlanɩ yemɔɩsɔ. Dɩ Jeju so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Nɩ cʋɛ wɩ wɩ der der paar kpalanyɔ yʋɔr yʋɔr.
42009015	Dɩ wɩ cʋʋ oti a cʋʋ wɩ fɛʋ dɩ wɩ der.
42009016	Dɩ Jeju gba buru yemɔɩɩle na thʋma yenyɔɔle, a gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ a bɩɛl Thãgba a pɛr, sa kuur buru a ha kpãkpãadara wɩ gba tɩnɛnɛ tibil jɔɔlera.
42009017	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ khor a hi phi; dɩ wɩ kɔɔ gbaar dakuruukɛ wɩ tɩnɛnɩ sa sɩ dɩɩ hi kpona yʋɔr yenyɔ.
42009018	Wi bɩɛl Jeju kɔɔ har dɩbara da-n bɩɛl Thãgba, dɩ a kɔɔ bulele ɔɔ kpãkpãadaraakɛ hanɩ kha na ɔr ayɩ: Amɛ tɩbɩla n yɩ mɩ dor?
42009019	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Ɩkhasɔ n yɩ Jã Batɩsɩtɩ fɩ do. Wɛ n yɩ Elɩ fɩ do. Wɛ n yɩ wo, mama Thãgbaa bobon bɩɛl ɩrɛ a the khirera.
42009020	Sɩ Jeju bule wi: Sɩ ner, amɛ nɩ-n yɩ mɩ dor? Dɩ Pɩɛr birsee: Thãgbaa Kirisiti fɩ do.
42009021	Sɩ Jeju kpãkpãa warɛ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka aa, wa-n so tibillə ga.
42009022	Dɩ a sor wo a ɓaan ayɩ: Dɔ mɛrkɛ dʋɔnnɩ tibili Bikuun n gaar bʋɔ jɔɔ. Dɩ kɔ̃tɩna, na bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na bo mer, sɩ dakha wa kʋ mɛr, sɩ wire yẽther wirera ma ɩɩrɛ na the khirera.
42009023	Agɩpɩ dɩ so war fɛʋ ayɩ: A ntɛ pɛr haar ɩna-n kpa mar, dɔ a faa dɩbara yɩrnanɛ, sɩ a gba ɔɔ kʋkʋ thɩr dɩwɩlʋ koo a na-n kpana mar.
42009024	Gɩdonɩ tibilikɛ n kanɩ dɩ hana bʋ dʋr na ɔɔ yi, ga ka na buurəəre. Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛɛ yi na bonɩ mɛrɛra, ɔr na 'lɛ gɩ waa gel.
42009025	Anyee bɔ ca ga taa tibil, ado a 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ sɩɩ do ɔɔ yi buurəəre, agɩbo dɩ kʋɛ ɔɔ dɩbara?
42009026	Dɩ a yicuru fʋ tibil mɛrɛra na ɩ̃ thɩmɩιra, yicuru na fʋrɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun ntɛra, ɔbɔɔkɛ ma birni na ɩ̃ na ɩ̃ i dʋbɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩɩda na dakha thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu phuusɔɔda.
42009027	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ɩkhasɔɔkɛ hanɩ kɩɛr na khiir sɩɩ do wa yɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar doaa ga.
42009028	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju mɩɩnɩ thɩmɩaakɛ pɩ dɩ a cʋʋ wire makõther, gɛr a kparɔ Pɩɛr na Jã na Jakɩ a jʋʋnna gɔ̃gʋɔna Thãgba bɩɛl paar.
42009029	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a hanɩ Thãgba bɩɛllɔ, ɔɔ ƴɛ debire dɩ ɔɔ kẽkẽ bulolo phõphõphõ dɩ a-n hɩl phalphalphal.
42009030	Dɩ hɩnɛ, tɩbɩla yenyɔ wɛ dɩ wa-n khʋɛ kha na ɔr. Mʋɩjɩ na Elɩ gɩ,
42009031	a the na carbararɛ, dɩ wa-n mɩɩ kha Jejuu khidaakɛ a na khini Jerujalɛm.
42009032	Sɩ daan kɔɔ fʋrɛ Pɩɛr na ɔɔ kpakpaarsɔ. Sɩ a wɩ jaa, wɩ yɩrɛ Jejuu carbara na tɩbɩla yenyɔɔle hanɩ kha na ɔr.
42009033	Ɔbɔɔle tɩbɩlaale n lɔrnɩ kʋɔn, Pɩɛr sor Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, gɩ bɔrɛ sɩ hanɩ kɩɛr. Sɩ dɔ waa yẽther, bɩɛl n do afɩda, bɩɛl n do Mʋɩjɩɩda, bɩɛl n do Elɩɩda. Gɩdonɩ aa jɩ gɩrɛ a-n sona'.
42009034	Dɩ mɔna a-n mɩɩnɩ thale, ndɔlɔ̃paar gbune a thi tɩbɩla yẽtheraale. Dɩ mɔna ndɔlɔ̃paarɩle n thi warnɩ, maar fʋlɛlɛ kpãkpãadara.
42009035	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ ther ndɔlɔ̃paarrara a so: Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mι phiirni. Na-n pιɛ nũu.
42009036	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ wι kɔɔ nιɛnι nʋɔɔle, Jeju sɛ dιbara. Dι kpãkpãadara pιrrɔrɛ, wa kɔɔ mιι tibil ga bɔɔle gιrɛ wι kɔɔ yιna'.
42009037	A dιι kɔɔ wιl wι ther gɔ̃gʋɔna dι wa-n gbũ, dι tibil jɔjʋɔ caan Jeju.
42009038	Dι hιnɛ, kũu bιɛl tibil jɔraale hulene: Dιιrdaar, mι-n phʋʋr fɛr hιnɛ mι bιsaanιkɛ, gιdonι ɔr dɔ ɩ̃ bikũu bιɛl.
42009039	Dι bɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuulera ιιrnaanι pι, dιι do dapaara a hulene, dι kɔ̃tɛɛbuurə n cʋgʋʋrɛ da-n laan da-n thena nyɔ̃thɩ̃ khɔrɔ̃ɔ. A ayι, ιnι-n thιιraarɛ kιɛr dιι do gbɔlɔlɔlɔ a sιraa waa dι ha.
42009040	Dι mι kɔɔ bιɛlɛ afι kpãkpãadara wι wea kɔ̃tɛɛbuurə, sι wa kɔɔ punoə'.
42009041	Dι Jeju so war: Nɛr nĩ babala na puu cʋʋdaraakɛɛ, ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ma thʋ̃ na toona nι gι dana? Dι ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ma thʋ̃ na fʋ nar haarrarakɛ gι dana? Kpa afι bikuunna a ɛna kɛ kιɛr.
42009042	Dι mɔ̃kɛ a-n wɔrɔnι, kɔ̃tɛɛbuurə gbaarɛ kpɛɛ da-n laan. Dι Jeju mananɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔlιle, sa kpɛɛ bιsaan a kpa ha ɔɔ thι.
42009043	Dι nʋɔ kpaa tιbιla fɛʋ mɔ̃ wι yιnι Thãgbaa puno hana. Mɔ̃kɛ nʋɔ kpaanι wɛr fɛʋ gιrɛra fɛʋʋkɛ Jeju cʋʋnι, a sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara:
42009044	Nι jιɛ pɛ ga thιmιιkɛ nũu bɔɔbɔɔ, gιdonι wa fʋrɛ mɛrkɛ dɔnι tibili Bikuun na ha tιbιla.
42009045	Sι ɔɔ kpãkpãadara na kɔɔ jι thιmιιrιle kιrʋa'. Gι kɔɔ ha warɛ gbul dι wa-n puno na jι kιrʋa', dι maar kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr dι wa bir 'la na bule ga.
42009046	Thɩ̃ banaa kɔɔ ιιrɛ awι thɩ̃thιιn, dι wa-n bana kha awι ha: Amɛ dɔ kɔ̃tιn gιrɛra asι thɩ̃thɩɩn ya fɛ?
42009047	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ jɩrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n kpɩɛrnɩ awɩ bɩnɔ, a kpa bɩsã buu pɔna dɩ khunəə sɩ dɩ so war:
42009048	Ntɛɛkɛ na teanɩ bɩsã buu thakɛ gɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ, mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ a tee, dɩ ntɛɛkɛ tea mɩnɩ, ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ a tee dakha. Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ da'lũu fɩɩʋ nɛrɛ fɛʋʋ thɩ̃thɩɩn, ɔr gɩɩkɛ kanɩ do kɔ̃tɩn.
42009049	Dɩ Jã so Jejura ayɩ: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ tibilikɛ n gbaannɩ afɩ i dɩ weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ da-n faa, dɩ sɩ kɔɔ pɩɛrʋʋ gɩdonɩ aa do asɩ kpakpaardaara'.
42009050	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Na-n pɩɛrʋa', gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n ƴaalɛ nɩnɩ sʋa', nɛrra a-n pɛ.
42009051	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wireekɛ Jeju teenanɩ a jʋnɛ ƴũ n thɔɔnɩ, Jerujalɛm a ga ƴɩɛ sa yɩ foo ɩnɩ-n thʋ le.
42009052	Dɩ a thʋɔn tɩbɩla, dɩ wɩ kɔɔ kʋʋlʋʋ ƴɩɛ a jal lõ Samarɩdaraa dɩ bɩɛlla wɩ gbɛbɩraa cɔ paar.
42009053	Sɩ dɩdaraale na kɔɔ tuə', gɩdonɩ Jerujalɛm khʋra a ga ƴɩɛ.
42009054	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara Jakɩ na Jã yɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ thale, wɩ buleele ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, fɩ-n ƴaalɛ sɩ wɛ dɔɔ gɩ the ƴũ gɩ gbũ gɩ hɩ̃ wɩ fɛʋ ya?
42009055	Dɩ Jeju kɩɩl a hɩɩn wɩ sa phaan wɩ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka [ayɩ: Na jɩɩ jɩ fɩl ca ʋrɛ nɩ hanana';
42009056	gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na ɩ̃ ɩ̃ cʋʋ tibil a jal bu paara', sɩ mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ taa tibil.] Sɩ agɩpɩ wɩ kɔɔ jaal dɩ kpɩɩ.
42009057	Mɔ̃kɛ wɩ kɔɔ hanɩ hʋɛra, tibil bɩɛl sor Jejura: Ma-n kpa farɛ paar wo paarɩkɛ fɩ-n jalnɩ.
42009058	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Bãɓoisɔ hananɛ awɩ ka, dɩ 'lominə hananɛ awɩ tɛl, sɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na hana kãkɛ ma jəəni yʋa'.
42009059	Sɩ a sor tibil bɩɛlla wo ayɩ: Na kpa mar. Dɩ birsee: Ha mɩ hʋɛ ɩ̃ jal ɩ̃ dʋ ɩ̃ thɩ ɓo.
42009060	Sɩ Jeju sʋʋraarɛ: Sɛ khesɔra wa-n dʋ awɩ khisɔ, sɩ fɛrɛ jala na mɩa Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda.
42009061	Dɩ bɩɛl wo sʋʋraa: Ma-n kpa farɛ Kɔ̃tιn, sι ha mι hʋɛ ɓo ɩ jal ɩ̃ fʋɔr ɩ̃ cɔdara wι tɔɔ bɔɔ.
42009062	Dι Jeju sʋʋraa: Tibil wo tibilikɛ fɔnι sũgbure da-n kʋʋl sι da-n hιιn khiro, a na mar na lõ Thãgba fãgadaarι dιra ga.
42010001	A gele ka pι, Kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ phiire kpãkpãadara kpalãther yʋɔr wo, a thɔ̃ wι yenyɔ yenyɔ ɔɔ ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ dɩɩra fɛʋ, na paar fɛʋʋkɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ teenanɩ a jala.
42010002	Sɩ a so warɛ: Jɔ jɔrɛ, sɩ jʋ kha na jɔra'. Gɛr gɩ na-n bɩɛlnɛ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn jʋ kharra, a thɔna thɔ̃dara wa-n kha jɔ.
42010003	Nɩ jala, sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, banaa nɩ ho dɩ ɩ̃ thɔ̃ kpesɔɔ thɩ̃thιιn.
42010004	Na-n fʋrɔ pɔtιma ga, na-n fʋrɔ kpakpaar lokaara', na-n fʋrɔ nɛfaa ga, dι na-n fʋɔr tibil hʋɛra ga.
42010005	Sι cʋɔr wo cʋɔrraakɛ na lonι, cacara nι kɔɔ sɔ: Ha ιι hana cʋɔrraakɛ.
42010006	Dι ado tibilikɛ dɔnι ha iedaar hale cʋɔrraale, anι ha ie na ɓaanaanɛ, a mɛ̃ gaa ga kɛrrɛ na bir nar.
42010007	Nι tɔɔ cɔ dɔɔraalera, dι gιrɛɛkɛ wa ha nιnι nι khɔ a na yɔna, gιdonι thɔ̃daar teenanɛ ɔɔ lɩmɩ. Na-n ιιr na kpaar cɔna cɔna ga.
42010008	Dι dιι wo dιιraakɛ na lonɩ dɩ wa tee nɩ, na-n khɔ dɩkor wo dɩkorɩkɛ wa ha nɩnɩ.
42010009	Na-n kpɛɛnɛ khodaraakɛ na hanɩle a na sɔna war: Bɔɔ n daan dɩ Thãgba na-n gba fãga nɛrɛra.
42010010	Sɩ dɩɩ wo dɩɩraakɛ na lonɩ kãkɛ wa tee nɩna', nɩ jala dɩ bɩnɔ a sɔ thakɛ ayɛwɔɔ:
42010011	Sɩ-n kpɛɛrɛ anɩ dɩ thɩlãkobiikɛ ma sɩnɩ nɛɛ dɩ sa-n faa nar, sɩ nɩ jɛrakɛ dɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do n daan.
42010012	Mɩ so narɛ wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla Sɔdɔmdaraa kɩɩlɩkɛ wa 'lɛnɩ na khɩɩr mɔ̃ dɩɩlee kɩɩl na khɩɩrna'.
42010013	Ga puu farɛ Korajɛ̃ dɩɩ. Ga puu farɛ Bɛcaɩda dɩɩ. Gɩdonɩ ado nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ cʋɛnɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ mɛ̃ Tιιr na Sιdɔ̃ dιιra, wa kɔɔ mãa debire haar kɛkɛkɛ sι na to bɔrɔ na bʋlna thoo.
42010014	Gɛr gι wireekɛ Thãgba na kιιlnanι tιbιla, Tιιrdara na Sιdɔ̃daraa kιιlιkɛ wa 'lɛnι na khιιr mɔ̃ anι kιιl na khιιrna'.
42010015	Sι fɛr Kapɛrnayʋm dιι, Thãgba na khəi fer na jʋʋnna ƴũ ya? Ǝ̃'ə̃, Thãgba na gbumo fer dι fa thʋ khĩdi dιι.
42010016	Tibilikɛ n pɛ nιnι nũu, mɛr a-n pɛ nũu. Tibilikɛ bɔ nιnι, mɛr a bo; dι tibilikɛ bɔ mιnι, ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mιnι a bo.
42010017	Dι kpalãther yʋɔr kɛrrɛ bir na daʋ dι wa-n so: Kɔ̃tιn, kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔrakɛ wι jo sarɛ dιι do afι i dɔ nɔɔ.
42010018	Dι Jeju so war: Mι kɔɔ torre Satana yire dι thena ƴũ a ji, mɔ̃kɛ thãgba n lenι dɔɔ.
42010019	Nι hιnɛ, mι ha nɛr punone dι na saarna siisɔ na lanasɔ na lãlaardaarι fãga fɛʋ, dι thɩ̃ bιɛllakɛ na puno na cʋʋ nι puurə'.
42010020	Sι na-n kãka thakɛ gιdonι kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ jo nara', sι nι ka na kãkanɛ gιdonι anι isɔ kherere Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
42010021	Ga bɔ bɩɛllaalera Jeju n kɔɔ kãkarɛ dɩɩ the Thu Phuurə da-n sona: Thɩrɛ, mɩ-n fʋɔr fɛr, fɛrkɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩra, gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ kɔɔ kernɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛra kpɛsɛdarara na thɩ̃ jɩnana, sa gba gɩ a nɩna bɩsã bii. Ɔɔ Thɩrɛ, fɛr gɩ kɔɔ da haar dɩ fɩ cʋʋ mɛ̃.
42010022	Ɩ̃ Thι gbaar thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ a ha mι, sι tibil na jι ntɛ Bikuun donι saagado Thιrɛ gaaga; dι tibil na jι dakha ntɛ Thιrɛ donι saagado Bikuun gaaga, saagado wo Bikuunna ɔr ƴaalɛ a nιrɔ ntaa ga.
42010023	Sι agιpι dι kɛr a telẽ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara a so war awι ha ayι: Gι da wιrɛraakɛ n yɛnι thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nι-n yιnι.
42010024	Gιdonι mι so narɛ, Thãgbaa bobona jɔɔ na fãgadarasɔ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wι yι gιrɛ nι-n yιnι sι wa kɔɔ yι ga, wι nιɛna dakha gιrɛɛkɛ nι-n nιnι sι wa kɔɔ nι ga.
42010025	Dι hιnɛ, jɔfʋ dιιrdaar bιɛl gι, a ιιr pɔ da-n fifilə Jeju, a bulee thakɛ: Dιιrdaar, anye ma cʋʋ a na 'lɛ yire khorr?
42010026	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Anye Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ so? Dɩ anye fɩ-n yɩ le?
42010027	Dɩ birsee: “Dɔ fa-n na Kɔ̃tɩn afɩ Thãgba na afɩ bɩ̃ fɛʋ, na afɩ ha fɛʋ, na afɩ fãga fɛʋ, na afɩ kpɩɛr fɛʋ, na afɩ 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃kɛ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara.”
42010028	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Fɩ ture dɩɩ bɔr, dɩ cʋɛ thalera fa 'lɛr yire.
42010029	Sɩ gɩdonɩ a-n kɔɔ ƴaalɛ a nɩna mɔ̃ a sarnɩ, a bulele Jeju: Dɩ amɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ 'walãkha tibililera?
42010030	Dɩ Jeju bir sʋʋraa wo ayɩ: Kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ the Jerujalɛm da-n jal Jeriko, a lõ yu hɔ̃hʋɔldarara dɩ wɩ tagɩrʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, sa bɩɩrʋʋ dɩ dã khir, sɩ dɩ wɩ fagʋʋ sa jal kɔ̃.
42010031	Dɩ dabɔɔlera, bonɩ jidaar bɩɛl kɔɔ gbaar ɔ hʋʋlera da-n jal, a phuro kuunnaale a golona ʋ̃ hʋ gɛl a jal.
42010032	Dɩ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ dɔnɩ Levɩɩ ca pɔr dakha a dã paarɩlera, a yɩ kuunile sa golona ʋ̃ hʋ gɛl a jal.
42010033	Sɩ Samarɩdaar bɩɛlɩkɛ n kpaarɛnɩ pɔr a dã kuunile. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a yɩɩnɩ, bʋɔ fʋʋrɛ.
42010034	Dɩ a tɔr pɔ dã a gba niin na taanɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ dɩvɛ̃, a pɩɛraa khoosɔra sa li. Agɩpɩ dɩ gbaa pɛ kũkəənə, a jalna kpakpal cɔ bɩɛlla da-n haan.
42010035	A dɩɩ wɩl, a tire wire yenyɔ thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ war a ha ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ kpakpal cɔ hɩɩndaar sa sʋʋraa: Gba na haanaa, sɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ fa kʋɛnɩ na dɛbɩrɔ, a mɩ bir ɩ̃ ma lɩmɩ fɛr.
42010036	Dɩ Jeju bulee: Ʋmɔ̃ wɛr yẽtherraale fɩ pɛr haar, ɔr dʋɔn 'walãkha tibil kuunnaakɛ lonanɩ yu hɔ̃hʋɔldarara?
42010037	Dɩ birsee: Ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dɔnaanɩ bʋɔ gɩ. Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dɩ fɛrɛ dakha jala na cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃.
42010038	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ Jeju hanɩ hʋɛra na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara dɩ wa-n jal, a lʋʋn dɩ bɩɛlla. Dɩ khɛ bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Martɩ teguure ɔɔ cɔ.
42010039	Dɩ Martɩɩ õkhɛrɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Marɩ toore Kɔ̃tɩnɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, da-n pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ nũu.
42010040	Sɩ Martɩ or har thɔ̃ jɔjʋɔra kĩkĩkĩ, sa gba pɔ Jejura a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ga ba fɩ gɩrɛɛkɛra ɩ̃ õkhɛr faa marnɩ thɔmaakɛra fɛʋ dɩbara gaa? Sʋɔraa a bulo mi.
42010041	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn birsee: Martɩ, Martɩ, fɩ-n dɛr dɩ fa-n jena thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔra.
42010042	Thɩ̃ bɩɛl dɩbara teana fɩ cʋʋrɛ. Marɩ kɔɔ phiire dabʋɔɔkɛ na hanɩ taa paara'.
42011001	Wi bɩɛl Jeju kɔɔ har pa bɩɛl da-n bɩɛl Thãgba. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a pɩnɩ, ɔɔ kpãkpãadaar bɩɛl sʋʋraarɛ aa: Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩrɛ sɩ sa-n bɩɛl Thãgba mɔ̃ Jã kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara.
42011002	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba nɩ sɔ thakɛ aa: Thɩrɛ, dɔ afɩ i n dʋbɩrɔ, dɔ afɩ fãgadaar do n ɩ̃.
42011003	Na hana sɩ wire fɛʋʋ dɩkookɛ na-n dana sɩnɩ.
42011004	Faa asɩ sopugosɔ a hana sɩ, gɩdonɩ sɛrɛ dakha sɩ-n faarɛ puureekɛ tɩbɩla n cʋʋ sɩnɩ dɩ sa-n ha wɩ. Dɩ fa-n faa sɩ fifiləle n puno sa'.
42011005	Dɩ Jeju so war wo: A tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn hana kuun a jal ɔɔ cɔ dɩnɩrɔ a sʋʋraa thakɛ: Ɩ̃ kuun, pema mɩ buru yẽther,
42011006	gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ kũu bɩɛl ther dɩkhãa pa a ɩ̃, sɩ ma hana thɩ̃ɛ a na haa ga.
42011007	Sɩ ole cɔ bɩnɔ birsee: Fa-n vɔɔ ma', loo khaanɛ pɩ dɩ ɩ̃ bɩsãsɔ na mɛrɛ sɩ phɩɩnɛ, ma puno na ɩɩr na ha fɩ gɩrɛ fɩ-n ƴaalna'.
42011008	Mɩ so narɛ, ga do a donɩ ɔɔ kuun, gɛr a na ɩɩrɔ na haa gɩrɛɛkɛ a-n ƴaalna', sɩ a na ɩɩrɛ na haa gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛra a-n ƴaalnɩ, gɩdonɩ ɔɔ kuun bɩɛlɛ da-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna.
42011009	Dɩ mɛrɛ, mɩ so narɛ: Na-n bɩɛlnɛ na 'lɛr, na-n ƴaalɛ na yɩɛrɛ, na-n bɛ loo wa khɛr nɛr.
42011010	Gɩdonɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n bɩɛlnɛnɩ a-n 'lɛr, ʋrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ a-n yɩɛrɛ, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n bɛnɩ loo wa khɛrʋʋrɛ.
42011011	Ʋmɔ̃ɔ thι anι thɩ̃thιιn ɔɔ bi na bιɛllɔ buru a haa bokaar? Agιbo dι bιɛlaa thʋm, sii a na haa gι do thʋm ya?
42011012	Dι a yɔl paar a bιɛl, laan a na haa ya?
42011013	Ado nɛrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnι tιι puusɔ jɩ thɩ̃ bʋɔ a na 'laa anι bisɔra, mɔ̃ ga thʋ̃ na da anι Thιraakɛ hanιle ƴũ na pɔna, da 'laa Thu Phuu na ha tιbιlaakɛ n bιɛlaanɩ?
42011014	Jeju weere kɔ̃tɛɛbu bɩɛlɩkɛ cʋɛnɩ kuun dɩ do nɔ madaar. Ɔbɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbuulera kɔɔ thɩɩraanɩ pɩ, nɔ madaar n mɩɩrɛ thɩmɩa dɩphã, dɩ nʋɔ kpaa tibil jɔɔle.
42011015	Sɩ wɩ̃ tibil wɛrra na-n so: Bɛljɛbulikɛ dɔnɩ yʋʋ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔra n hanaa fãga dɩ weena kɔ̃tɛɛbii.
42011016	Wɩ̃ tibil wo na-n fifiləə a bulee nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ thãgbara ƴũ.
42011017	Mɔna Jeju jɩnɩ awɩ kpɩɛr a so warɛ: Fãgadaar dɩ wo fãgadaar dɩɩkɛ n tɩnɛnɛnɩ a bir da-n kena dɩbara a na wɩɛlɛ, dɩ cɔna dakha na wɩɛlɛ kpa kha kpa kha.
42011018	Dɩ gɛr gι, a Satã tɩnɛ a bir da-n kena dɩbara, mɔ̃ ɔɔ fãgadaar dɩ na fʋ sɩ na jɩɩl, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n sor: Bɛljɛbul hana mɩ fãga dɩ ma-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ?
42011019	Dɩ ado mɛrɛ, Bɛljɛbuli fãga mɩ-n gba dɩ ma-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ, sɩ anɩ bɩsãsɔ amɛɛ i wɩ-n gba dɩ wa-n weena wɩ? Dɩ gɛr gɩ wɛr thɛthɛra na dʋɔn anɩ so kɩɩldara.
42011020	Sɩ ado Thãgbaa fãga mɩ-n gba dɩ ma-n weena kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ, ga dor Thãgbaa fãgadaar do dã nɛr mɛ̃ dɩphã.
42011021	A kũu khɩɩ hana ko ke thɩ̃ɛ a na bɛrna ɔɔ cɔ, gɩrɛɛkɛ a hɩnɩ na toore bɔɔbɔɔ.
42011022	Sɩ ado bɩɛlɩkɛ hananɩ fãga a jʋɔ pɔr a punoo, a na fʋʋrɛ sɩ na taa ɔɔ ko ke thɩ̃sɔɔkɛra fɛʋ a-n kɔɔ kpɩɛrɔnɩ, sɩ a tɩnɛ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a kɔɔ taaraanι.
42011023	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n hanɩ kha na mɛrɛa', ɩ̃da a-n bo; dɩ wo ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n bulo mini sɩ kpa ga, ɔr n bɩ̃bιlanɛ gι.
42011024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl n thenι tibillə, a-n jaal da-n kpaar bəənnə da-n ƴaal kãkɛ a na toonι na hιιr. A a na yι ga, a-n sor dι yι: Ma kɛrrɛ na bir ɩ̃ cɔ kãkɛ mι kɔɔ thenι.
42011025	A a pɔ dã a yι cʋɔrιle dι wι kpabι a gbɛbιrι thɩ̃ɛ bɔɔbɔɔ;
42011026	le a-n jal dιphã mɛ̃ dι kpa kɔ̃tɛɛbi kpιιsɔ wo makonyɔɔkɛ n hʋɔlɛnι dι wι jʋɔ, dι wι pɔ a lõ a too le. Dι mɔ̃ gι hanι kuunnaale pιpιι paar, gι ka puurore a jɔ caca fʋ paar.
42011027	Dι mɔ̃kɛ Jeju kɔɔ mιιnι thale, khɛ bιɛl tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thιιn sʋʋraarɛ na nɔ kheu: Gι da khɛrraakɛ kɔna fɩnɩ na ɩlɛ̃sɔɔkɛ fɩ mamɩnɩ.
42011028	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Ɔɔ, ga ka na dar wɩrɛraakɛ n pɛnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ nũu dɩ wa-n cʋʋ.
42011029	Mɔna tibil jɔɔle kpanɩ dɩ wa-n jɛ, le Jeju ma da-n so: Nĩdaraakɛ dʋɔn tɩɩ puusɔɔkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ. Sɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kpɩɩ na bir na yɩ saagado Jonasɩɩda gaaga.
42011030	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ Jonasɩ kɔɔ donɩ jɩɩn Nɩnɩvɩdarara, mɛna mɛr tibili Bikuun na do jɩɩn nĩdararaakɛ dakha.
42011031	Wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, khɛr fãgadaarɩkɛ kɔɔ hanɩ wi phã paar nyɔ̃bɩlana, na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera nakha nĩdaraakɛ, dɩ ɔr na heene wɩ sor. Gɩdonɩ ɔr, thɩ khu paar a kɔɔ the a pɔ a pɛ Salomɔ̃ɔ kpɛsɛ nũu. Sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, ʋkhaakɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ Salomɔ̃ hakɛ.
42011032	Wireekɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla, Nɩnɩvɩdara na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera nakha nĩdaraakɛ, dɩ wɛr na heene wɩ sor, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ debire haar ɔbɔɔkɛ Jonasɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ. Sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, ʋkhaakɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ Jonasɩ hakɛ.
42011033	Tibil na gbaar lãphã a na pɛ wo sɩ a ker ya, agɩbo a suuro bɩlãkpʋʋn ya? Ga do bilela a na dɛ̃ɛ dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ n lonanɩ le n yɩ dahɩraa?
42011034	Afɩ yi dʋɔn lãphã afɩ tomɩra, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ afɩ yi bɔrnɩ, afɩ tomɩ fɛʋ dahɩrɛra gɩ-n ha. Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ afɩ yi na bɔrna', afɩ tomɩ fɛʋ dabirəra gɩ-n ha.
42011035	Gɛr gɩ na jɩɛ hɩɩn dɩ dahɩrɛɛkɛra fɩ hananɩ afɩ bɩnɔ, ga-n do dabirə ga.
42011036	Sɩ ado afɩ tomɩ fɛʋ har dahɩrɛra, dɩ kho bɩɛl na bo too dabirəra ga, ga dor a har dahɩrɛra fɛʋ gɩ ho mɔ̃ lãphã n carã fɩnɩ ɔɔ hɩrɛ.
42011037	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju mɩɩnɩ pɩ, jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar bɩɛl wɩɩrɛ a pɔ ɩnɩ cɔ a khɔ dɩkor. Dɩ jal lõ dɩko kho paar.
42011038	Dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaarɛ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaarɩle, mɔ̃kɛ a yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do Jeju na kɔɔ phʋɔl dɩbara ɓo sɩ da-n kho dɩkora'.
42011039	Sɩ Kɔ̃tɩn sʋʋraarɛ: Nɛr jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara, nɩ-n cɔcɔɔrɛ thɩ̃ yɔdaa khiru na dɩko khodaa khiru, sɩ bɩnɔ nɩ hinəne thɩ̃ tagɩrɩ kpɩɛrɛ na dakha kpallɛ.
42011040	Də̃bələ ha nɩ bã, ga do ʋrɛɛkɛra cʋɛnɩ khiru, ɔrra cʋɛ bɩnɛ dakha gaa?
42011041	Nɩ ka na 'laanɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ hanɩ bɩnɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na do daphuu nɛrɛra.
42011042	Sɩ ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n tire bɩɛl yʋɔr anɩ bi fara na anɩ thɩ̃ phulosɔraakɛ fɛʋ dʋɔnnɩ bii. Sɩ dɩ nɩ hɛbɩ fɩl sarʋ na naʋʋkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Thãgbaada. Sɩ gɛr ka do thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ teananɩ na-n cʋɛ, sɩ ga do wɩ yɩ nɩ hɛba gela'.
42011043	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n nar ƴɛ kʋʋl too paar Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ. Nɩ-n nar dakha wo tɩbɩla na-n fʋɔrɛ nɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋ ƴatɔɔsɔ.
42011044	Nɛrɛ ga puu narɛ, gɩdonɩ nɩ hʋrɛ kaakɛ tɩbɩla n saarnɩ, gɩdonɩ ga yɩr dɩ wɩ jɩ kaa ga.
42011045	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar bɩɛl sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar, thalera fɩ-n mɩɩnɩ, sɛr fɩ-n nɩɩr dakha.
42011046	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Nɛr jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ ga puu narɛ dakha, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n heene tɩbɩla heendaasɔɔkɛ dɩbarɔnɩ, sɩ wo na-n thar heendaasɔrara na nyɔ̃ɔ fɩɩʋraka'.
42011047	Nɛrɛ ga puu narɛ, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n mɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔkɛ anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ kʋʋrnɩɩ ka.
42011048	Nɛr dʋɔn wɩrɛ n nɛnanɩ mɔ̃ anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ thɔna hanɩ, dɩ nɩ tu ger gɩdonɩ wɛr, wɛr kɔɔ kʋʋrɛ Thãgbaa bobonasɔ. Sɩ nɛrɛ, nɛr n mɛ awɩ kasɔ.
42011049	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa so ayɩ: Ma thɔ̃ warɛ bobonasɔ na thɔ̃thɔnasɔ. Wa kʋʋrɛ wɛ wɛrra, dɩ ɩkhasɔ wa hʋɔl warɛ.
42011050	Gɛrra na dɔ nɔɔ dɩphã dɩ sor na heen nĩdaraakɛ Thãgbaa bobonasɔ fɛʋʋ tɔmιnaakɛ wι kɔɔ deernι kɛkɛkɛ dιι fʋna thιιkɛɛ ti bɔɔ,
42011051	Abɛlι tɔmɩ̃ gι fʋna a dana Jakarιιda, kɛ wι kɔɔ kʋnι bonι ji paar na Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ thɩ̃thιιn. Ɔɔ mι so narɛ, sor na heene nĩdaraakɛ gι do tιbιla fɛʋʋlee tɔmɩ̃ dɔ nɔɔ.
42011052	Ga puu narɛ nɛr jɔfʋ dιιrdarasɔ, gιdonι nι tire lakileekɛ n khɛranι jιιr, dι anι thɛthɛ na-n lona', wιrɛ n ƴaalɛnι wι lõ na-n sι war wo wι lona ga.
42011053	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju thenι paarιle, jɔfʋ dιɩrdarasɔ na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ mar dɩ wa-n gbʋɔrʋʋ na nĩkhii, gɩ cʋgʋʋ a mɩɩ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔjɔɔ;
42011054	gɩdonɩ wɩ nʋɔrɛ wɩ fʋʋ dɩkhaa thɩmɩɩraakɛ na thɛnɩ ɔɔ nɔɔ.
42012001	Ɔbɔɔlera tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ kpa a jɛ jɛ paar gbɩlanɩ tə̃tə̃tə̃ a thʋ̃ dɩ wa-n saar kha, dɩ Jeju ma da-n so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara caca ayɩ: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔɔ tabɩraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩnɛ yenyɔ fɩlɛ.
42012002	Thɩ̃ɛ na hale na ker sɩ ga do wɩ cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ thaa ga, dɩ thɩ̃ɛ na hale a na ha gbul sɩɩ do wa jɩ gaaga.
42012003	Dɩ gɛr gɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na mɩɩnɩ pa birə paar, dahɩrɛra wa nɩ gɩ, dɩ gɩrɛ na bʋ̃bʋʋnɩ du bɩnɔ, nãsʋrɔ wa hulẽ gi.
42012004	Mɩ so narɛ nɛrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ ɩ̃ kuunsɔ: Na-n ma wɩrɛɛkɛ n kɔnɩ tomɩr, sɩ agɩpɩ wa-n puno cʋʋ dɩkha ɓaan bãa ga.
42012005	Ma nɩ narɛ ntɛɛkɛ nɩ teenanɩ na-n ma. Na-n ma ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ punone a a kʋ pɩ, sɩ dɩ dʋna dɔɔra. Ɔɔ mɩ so narɛ, ɔr gɩɩkɛ teananɩ na-n ma.
42012006	Ga do war be yenã wɩ-n dolõ 'lominə yemɔɩaa? Sɩrakɛ bɩɛl na hale dɩ Thãgba na diinə ga.
42012007	Dɩ anɩ yʋsũsɔrakɛ, Thãgba ther ger fɛʋ. Gɛr gɩ na-n do maar na-n fʋ na', anɩ the nɔ khɩɩrɛ a jɔ 'lomĩ jɔjɔjʋɔ.
42012008	Sɩ mɩ so narɛ, tibil wo tibilikɛ n tuon mini tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra, mɛr tibili Bikuun na tuure dakha Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔ ƴɛra.
42012009	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ bɔ mɩnɩ tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra, ma bor ntɛɛle dakha Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔ ƴɛra.
42012010	Dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na mɩanɩ thɩmɩɩ puu na pɛ mɛr tibili Bikuunna, Thãgba na faarɛ ga sopugo caale na ha ntɛ. Sɩ tibilikɛ na kʋɛanɩ Thu Phuu i, Thãgba na faa ga sopugo caale kpɩɩraka'.
42012011	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wa kpa nɩnɩ wa-n jalna kɩɩl paar Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnana, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔ ƴɛra, na fãgadarasɔɔ ƴɛra, na-n hana dɛ mɔ̃kɛ na mɩɩnɩ gɩ taa na', agɩbo gɩrɛɛkɛ na sona';
42012012	gɩdonɩ Thu Phuu na dɩrɛ nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ teananɩ sor dɩ na so dabɔɔlera.
42012013	Dɩ kũu bɩɛl tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thɩɩn sor Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, sɔ ɩ̃ õkuunna sɩ tɩnɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ asɩ thɩ khini sa faa sar, dɩ Jeju birsee:
42012014	Kuun, amɛ kɔɔ pɛ mar ɩ̃ dɔ anɩ so gʋʋrdaar agɩbo anɩ khĩdi thɩ̃ tɩnɛdaar?
42012015	Agɩpɩ dɩ so war: Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ ha pɩɛr caarsɔra dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ, gɩdonɩ tibil na puno na 'lɛ yire ɔɔ lẽle thɩ̃ jɔ hanana ga, a a lerakɛ dɩɩ ha mɔ̃.
42012016	Dɩ a so warɛ sokpaakɛ ayɩ: Lẽle kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hale dɩ thɩ̃ɛ bʋɔraa lɔɔ dɩɩ ka.
42012017	Dɩ a kpɩɛrɛ ɔɔ hara sa so: Anye ma cʋʋ ya fɛ? Gɩdonɩ ma hana thʋ̃ khɩɩ a na urro ɩ̃ jʋ bã.
42012018	Sι agιpι dι so: Hιnɛ gιrɛ ma cʋʋnι dιphã. Ma tʋɔrɛ ɩ̃ thʋ̃sɔ a na kpɛɛ, sι ɩ̃ bir ɩ̃ mι dakɔ̃tιna gι jɔ mɛ̃; agιpι le ma ur ɩ̃ jʋ ɩ̃ thιιnna ɩ̃ lẽle thɩ̃sɔ fɛʋ.
42012019	Dι ma sor ɩ̃barara nayι: Mɛrɛ, mι hananɛ lẽle thɩ̃ɛ a thιιn dιι jɔr a na cʋʋ yɛna jɔɔjɔɔ. Ma toore ma-n hɩɩr ɩ̃ kho ma-n yɔna ma-n kãkana.
42012020	Sɩ Thãgba sʋʋraa: Fɛr də̃bəəlu, nĩ dιtιnɔɔkɛ ma teere afι thu, sι gιrɛɛkɛra fɛʋ fι kɔɔ gbɛbιnι amɛɛda ga do wo?
42012021	Mɛ̃ gι ha na tibilikɛ n thιnɛnι thɩ̃ɛ gι dɔ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛda, sι dιι do Thãgbaa pa wer, aa do lẽledaara'.
42012022	Agιpι Jeju sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Gɛr gι dι ɩ̃ so nar ayι: Na-n dɛ anι yirə dιko thιmιιrra, anye na kho yaa, dι tomιrιdara gι, anye na to yaa ga.
42012023	Gιdonι yire dor thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι a jɔ dιkor, dι tomιr dakha dor thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι a jɔ kɩ̃kιιn.
42012024	Na-n kpιɛrna 'lominəsɔ na hιnɛ, wa-n diirə', wa-n kha ga, wa-n hana dιko thιιn paar dι thʋnɛ ga, sι Thãgba n haanɛ wι. Anι the nɔ ga khιιr a jɔ 'lominəəda fĩiəə?
42012025	Amɛ nɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thιιn na punone a na tɔ ɔɔ yɛ nɔ na dɛɛnɔ dɛrra?
42012026	Dι mɔ̃ na-n marnι na cʋʋrakɛ thɩ̃ buə', sι mɔ̃gιdo dι na-n dɛna gιrɛɛkɛ sɛnι?
42012027	Na-n kpιɛrna naporsɔ wo na hιnɛ mɔ̃kɛ wι-n phuni. Wa-n kpar kẽkẽ wiirə', wa-n le kẽkena ga. Sι mι so narɛ Salomɔ̃ɔ thɛthɛrakɛ kɛ dɔnι fãgadaar, na ɔɔ nyɔ̃kor bɔ fɛʋ, aa kɔɔ to kɩ̃kιιn dιι ho wɛr bιɛllaka'.
42012028	Dɩ a Thãgba to hʋɔnɩkɛ hanɩle hʋɔnɔ nĩ dɩɩ ha thaa, sɩɩ do cʋɔ wa to garɛ dɔɔ, a na ka na cʋʋ mɛ̃ nɛrɛra dakha gaa, nɛrɛɛkɛ kanɩ hana ha pɛrɛ gbe?
42012029	Dɩ nɛrɛ na-n ƴaal gɩrɛ na khonɩ na gɩrɛ na yɔna', dɩ na-n too na dɛdɛda'.
42012030	Gɩdonɩ gele fɛʋ wɩrɛ na jɛnɩ Thãgba ga n ƴaalɛ gι, sι ado nɛr gι, anɩ Thɩ jɩrɛ gɩrɛ n ɓɔra nɩnɩ.
42012031	Sɩ nɩ ka na ƴaalɛ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do, sɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera fɛʋ Thãgba na ha nɛr na ɓaan.
42012032	Ɩ̃ bana bi, na-n do maar n fʋ na', gɩdonɩ anɩ Thɩra gɩ da dɩ na ha nɩ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩ.
42012033	Nɩ dolone anɩ lẽle thɩ̃sɔ a na hana bɔdara. Nɩ yɩrana mũsũ lokanaakɛ na kʋɛana', na lẽle thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, kɛ na dɔnɩ dapɩnana', kãkɛ yu na dana', dɩ ɔphãkerẽsɔ wɛ a na kʋɛ ga.
42012034	Gɩdonɩ kãkɛ anɩ lẽle thɩ̃sɔ hanɩ, le anɩ ha na ha dakha.
42012035	Nɩ gbɛbɩrɛ anɩ dɩbara a cʋɛ anɩ lãphãsɔ ga-n hɩrɛ.
42012036	Dɩ nɛrɛ, nɩ hɔ tɩbɩlaakɛ tɔɔnɩ dɩ wa-n pɩɛr awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ na thɛnɩ herra na ɩ̃, wɩ khɛrʋʋ loo khə̃khə̃ ɔbɔɔkɛ a na danɩ a na-n be.
42012037	Ga dar thɔ̃darasɔraale, a awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na pɔ a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa jʋʋr. Sobɔr mɩ so nar, a na gbɛbɩrɛ ɔɔbara sa cʋʋ wɩ wɩ too dɩko kho paar, a tɔ a pɔ a na-n tɩnɛ wɩ.
42012038	Ga dar thɔ̃darasɔraale na ka, ado awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na ɩ̃ a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa jʋʋr thakɛ, a dɩnɩrɔ gɩ, a yɔl ko khɩɩ bɔɔ gɩ.
42012039	Nɩ jɩɛ jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ bɔɔbɔɔ, ado cɔdaar kuun jɩrɛ bɔɔkɛ yu na pɔnɩ ɔɔ cɔ, a na-n bɛrɛ a na sɩɩraa a lʋ̃ʋ cʋɔrɔa'.
42012040	Nɛrɛ dakha nι gbɛbɩrɛ pɛ, gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na bire na ɩ̃ bɔɔkɛ na kpɩɛrna gɩna'.
42012041	Dɩ Pɩɛr bule: Kɔ̃tɩn, sɛr fɩ-n sor sokpaakɛra yaa, agɩbo tɩbɩla fɛʋra gɩ?
42012042	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn birsee: Ʋmɔ̃ dʋɔn thɩ̃ hɩɩndaarɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ sobɔ cʋʋdaar, kɛ kpɛsɛnɛnι, dι ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na pɛr da do ɔɔ cɔdaraa hιιndaar a na-n hana wι dιkɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ gι teenanι?
42012043	Ga dar thɔ̃daar ca olela ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na-n danι a yιι a na-n cʋʋ mɛ̃.
42012044	Sobɔr mι so nar, ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na jιɛ cʋgʋʋ da do hιιndaar ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔra fɛʋ.
42012045	Sι ado thɔ̃daarιle sor ɔɔbarara ayι: Ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ n pʋɔrɛ, sa ma da-n bɩɩr thɔ̃daar kona na thɔ̃daar khɛra, dι khona da-n yɔna dɩ taan na-n kʋʋ;
42012046	thɔ̃daarɩlee kɔ̃tɩ̃ na phurore dawiikɛ aa-n pɩɛrʋʋna', na bɔɔraakɛ aa kpɩɛrnana'. Dɩ a na cɩɩrɛ yιra yιra, sι na gbaa na pɛ wιrɛraakɛ na pιɛrnɩ haara'.
42012047	Thɔ̃daarɩkɛ kɔɔ jɛnɩ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ tuur sɩ aa gbɛbɩ thɩ̃a', agɩbo aa cʋʋ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ n ƴaalna', a na 'lɛr bɩɩrɛ dɩ a kɔ̃tɩ̃ na sobɔr.
42012048	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na jɛna', sa cʋʋ gɩrɛɛkɛ dananɩ bɩɩrɛ, a na 'lɛ bɩɩrɛ jɔa'. Tibilikɛ wɩ hanɩ jɔɔ, mɛ̃ wa bulee jɔɔ dakha, na tibilikɛ wɩ pɛrnɩ a na-n hɩnɛ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ, mɛ̃ wa bulee a na kpãkpaanɔ jɔɔ.
42012049	Dɔɔ mɩ ɩna ɩ̃ pɛ thɩɩra, dɩ anye mɩ-n ƴaal 'lo a gɩ 'li mar?
42012050	Mɩ teenanɛ ɩ̃ 'lɛ yɔ kpɛɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ bʋɔɔkɛ ma gaarnɩ, sɩ nɩ yɛ mɔ̃ gɩ do marnɩ kpɩɛrɛɛkɛ n 'waan mɩnɩ ɓoɓo phaphapha gɩ dã.
42012051	Nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ ha ɩɩ mɩ ɩna ɩ̃ 'laa thɩɩra gaa bɛ? Ǝ̃'ə̃, mɩ so narɛ leere gɩ.
42012052	Gɩdonɩ a fʋna nɛnɛ̃kɛ, tɩbɩla yemɔɩ cɔ bɩɛlla na leere kha. Yẽther na yenyɔ na ti kha dɔa', dɩ yenyɔ na yẽther dakha na ti kha dɔa'.
42012053	Thɩrɛ na ti kha dɔɔ na ɔɔ bikuuna', dɩ bikuun na ti kha dɔɔ na ɔɔ thɩ dakha ga. Nɩrɛ na ti kha dɔɔ na bikhɩɛna', dɩ bikhɩɛn na ti kha dɔɔ na nɩrɛ dakha ga. Nɩrɛ na ti kha dɔɔ na ɔɔ bikuuni khɛra', dɩ bikuuni khɛr na ti kha dɔɔ na ɔɔ koo nɩ dakha ga.
42012054	Dɩ Jeju sor tibil jɔraale wo ayɩ: Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ ndɔlɔ̃paar gananɔ dɩɩ birə, mee nɩ-n sor dapaara dɩ nɩ yɩ, thãgba nyʋɔn na daan, dɩɩ dã ger oti.
42012055	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ jɩɛ dɩ ga-n the wi phã paar nyɔ̃bɩlana, nɩ-n sor dɩ nɩ yɩ aa: Susuur na kʋrɛ, dɩɩ dã ger oti.
42012056	Nɛr bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, nɩ-n punone dɩ nɩ jɩ mɔ̃kɛ thɩ̃ɛ n hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩra, sɩ mɔ̃ na-n ka dɩ nɩ jɩ mɔ̃ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ wer hana?
42012057	Dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n ka nɩ jɩ anɩbara gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dasarʋa?
42012058	Ado afɩ sodaar we fɩ kɩɩl paar kɔ̃tɩnaa ƴɛra, ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ hanɩ jaal na afɩ sodaarra, dɔ bʋɔ sɩ nɩ gʋʋr kha sorra gɩ pɩ le hʋɛra; agado mɛ̃ gaa, a na jalna fɛr so kɩɩldaarɩ ƴɛra, dɩ so kɩɩldaar dakha na gba fɩ a na ha gardɩ, dɩ gardɩ na khaan fɩ khaɩra.
42012059	Sɩ mɩ so farɛ, fa the le kpɩɩraka', phaphapha fɩ lɩmɩ gɩ pɩna.
42013001	Ga bɔraalera wɩ̃ tibilsɔ kɔɔ pɔr a mɩɩ Jeju gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananɩ Galiledaraakɛ Pɩlatɩ kɔɔ kʋʋrnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ bonɩ jiro.
42013002	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ dɩ Galileda wele kɔɔ dʋɔn sopugodara a jɔ wɩ̃ Galiledarasɔ fɛʋ, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ gaarɛ bʋɔ thalaa bɛ?
42013003	Ǝ̃'ə̃, mɩ so narɛ, ga do mɛ̃ ga; nɛrɛ dakha ado na debi haara', mɛna na khiir fɛʋ.
42013004	Dɩ agɩbo tɩbɩla yʋɔr makõtherɩkɛ cɔ gbãakɛ hanɩ Siloe kɔɔ jironi a kʋʋr, nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ dɩ wɛr kɔɔ dʋɔn sopugodara a jɔ Jerujalɛmdara fɛʋaa bɛ?
42013005	Ǝ̃'ə̃, mɩ so narɛ, ga do mɛ̃ ga; nɛrɛ dakha, ado na debi haara', mɛna na khiir fɛʋ.
42013006	Dɩ Jeju so warɛ sokpaakɛ ayɩ: Kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hana thɩrʋ ɔɔ lɔɔ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ se bɔɔ danɩ, a pɔr a khʋ̃, aa yɩɩraa thɩ̃a'.
42013007	Dɩ a sor ɔɔ lɛ hɩɩndaarra: Hɩnɛ, yɛna yẽther ha gɩrɛ mɩ ɩnɩ kɛ a ƴaal ɩ̃ khʋ̃ be, sɩ ma yɩ thɩ̃a'. Kuro kpɛa. Anye a na harɔ kɛ a na-n kʋɛ thɩɩ mɔlɔ?
42013008	Dɩ ɔɔ lɛ hɩɩndaar birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩɛraa dɛʋʋkɛ wo, ɩ̃ cɩɩn ɩ̃ finə sɩ ɩ̃ pɛr beethɩn;
42013009	agakpaana a na ser na yɩɛrɩkɛ na ɩnanɩ, sɩ ado aa sa', fɩ kur dɩphã fɩ kpɛɛ.
42013010	Hɩɩr wi bɩɛl, Jeju kɔɔ hale Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ bɩɛlla da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla.
42013011	Dɩ hɩnɛ, khɛ bɩɛl gɩ, a halera dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbuu hanaa a pɩɛraa taan kɛkɛkɛ, dɩ cʋʋna yɛna yʋɔr makõther. A khar, aa kɔɔ puno na 'lamɩsɛ kpɩɩ bã.
42013012	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju yɩɩnɩ, a wɩɩrɛ dɩ pɔ dɩ sʋʋraa ayɩ: Khɛr, fɩ 'lɛr taarɛ afɩ tanaakɛra fɩ hananɩ.
42013013	Agɩpɩ Jeju dɛɛnaa nyɛ̃ɛ; dɩ dapaara dɩ 'lamɩsɛ, da-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i.
42013014	Sɩ nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋrɛ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, gɩrɛraakɛ Jeju kpɛɛnɩ khɛrɩle hɩɩr wire. Dɩ a sor tibil jɔraale: Wire maadõ hale kɛ dʋɔnnɩ thɔ̃ do wire, gɛr gɩ nɩ ɩna wa-n kpɛɛ nɩ khoo ga wisɔraale. Sɩ na-n do ga-n do hɩɩr wirə'.
42013015	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn birsee: Nɛr bɩnɛ yenyɔdara, nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl na-n khɛr anɩ nake, agɩbo anɩ kũkə̃ hɩɩr wire na barana a jalna dɩ yɔ nyʋɔnaa?
42013016	Sɩ khɛrɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Abɩrahamɩ bikhɛrɩkɛ Satã kɔɔ lini ɩɩrɔ kɛkɛkɛ dɩ cʋʋna yɛna yʋɔr makõther, ga teena gɩ do hɩɩr wire mɩ thʋbʋʋ lirikɛra gaa?
42013017	Mɔna a-n mιɩnɩ gele, yicuru fʋrɛ ɔɔ sodarasɔ fɛʋ, sɩ dɩ tibil jɔɔle wer na-n kãka nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔraakɛ fɛʋ a-n cʋʋnɩ.
42013018	Jeju bire so war wo: Anye Thãgbaa fãgadaar do hona, dɩ anye ma gba a na mɩɛna ya fɛ?
42013019	Gɩ hʋrɛ seneve bireekɛ n hanɩ fɩɩʋ, kɛ kuun kɔɔ gbanɩ a jal ɔɔ nãkʋɔrra, dɩɩ phu a ɩɩr a do thɩrʋ, dɩ 'lominə na-n tɛl ɔɔ jɛ̃sɔra.
42013020	A bire so war wo: Anye ma gba na mɩɛna mɔ̃ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do hanɩ ya fɛ?
42013021	Gɩ hʋrɛ tabɩɩrɩkɛ khɛr kɔɔ gbanɩ a mʋʋ buru mɩ̃ nyɔ̃kpõ khaa yẽtherra, phaphapha dɩ buru mɩ̃ boloola fɛʋ bʋ̃.
42013022	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ kpaarɛ dɩ kɔ̃tɩnana na dɩ biisɔra a dɩɩr tιbιla da-n jalna Jerujalɛm.
42013023	Dι tibil bιɛl bulee: Kɔ̃tιn, sιι do tιbιla gbe 'lɛr taarɛ bɛ? Dι Jeju birse wi:
42013024	Nι yιra lonana lõfonʋɔɔkɛ 'luruneni, gιdonι mι so narɛ, tιbιla jɔɔ na ƴaalɛ wι lõ sι wa punoə'.
42013025	Gιdonι ɔbɔɔkɛ cɔdaar kuun na ιιrnι na khaan loo na pι, sι dι na pɔ na jιιl phiilo, le na ma na-n be loo na-n sona: Kɔ̃tιn, khɛra sι loo. Dι a na birse ner: Ma jι kãkɛ nι thena'.
42013026	Dι mɛ̃ na ma na-n so: Sι kɔɔ khor dι sa-n yɔna afι ƴɛ thɩ̃thιιn, dι fι kɔɔ dιιr sɛr dakha asι dʋɔ.
42013027	Sι a na birse ner nayι: Ma jι kãkɛ nι thena'. “Nι tɔ jala mι ƴɔɔ, nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n cʋɛnι gιrɛ na-n sarana'.”
42013028	Dɩ le na bɩ na-n yɩrna nyɩma ɔbɔɔkɛ na yɩnɩ Abɩraham, na Ɩjakɩ, na Jakɔbɩ, na Thãgbaa bobonasɔ fɛʋ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra, sɩ dɩ wa faa ne wer phiilo.
42013029	Tɩbɩla na ther wi phã paar, na wi lõ paar, na gɛlʋ yenyɔra fɛʋ, a na too dɩko kho paar Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
42013030	Sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ sɩka pɩra, wɛr na fien na do ƴɛ kʋla, sɩ ƴɛ kʋla n fi wɩ do sιka pιra.
42013031	Ga bɔɔlera ιkhaa jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ pɔ a so Jejura: Ɩrɛ thɛ kιɛrra, gιdonι Ɛrɔɔdι n ƴaalɛ a kʋ fι.
42013032	Dι birse wi: Nι jala sɔ fιfιllaalera ayɛ: Hιnɛ, nĩ na cʋɔ ma weere kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ a na kpɛɛna khodarasɔ, sι ɩ̃ thɔ̃ na pιrɛ balãther wire.
42013033	Sι nĩ na cʋɔ na gιbɩ̃ι, gι teenanɛ ɩ̃ gba ɩ̃ hʋ ma-n jal, gιdonι Thãgbaa bobon na teena a khe a hʋnɔna Jerujalɛm dιa'.
42013034	Jerujalɛm, Jerujalɛm, fɛrkɛ n kʋrɛnι Thãgbaa bobona, dι fa-n dʋʋrna wιrɛɛkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ thɔ̃ farnι bokana, balamɔ̃ balamɔ̃ mι kɔɔ ƴaal ɩ̃ gbɛbιra afι too mɔ̃kɛ yɔl nιι n gbɛbιnι ɔɔ bisɔ dι thiro gbɛla, sι na kɔɔ tuə'.
42013035	Nι hιnɛ, wa faa narɛ anι cɔra dι ga do cɔ kpoloo. Sι mι so narɛ ayι, na yι mι bã phaphapha gι dana bɔɔkɛ na sonι nayι: “Ʋrɛ n ιnanι na Kɔ̃tιnι i hιna khιιrɛ.”
42014001	Hιιr wi bιɛl Jeju kɔɔ lʋʋn jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιɛlι cɔ a kho dιkor. Dι wιrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hanιle n kɔɔ jʋrʋʋrɛ.
42014002	Dι hιnɛ, kũu bιɛl gι, a hale Jejuu ƴɛra a hana khookɛ n 'laanɛnι tomι mʋɔrɛ.
42014003	Dι Jeju bule jɔfʋ dιιrdara na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ ayι: Hιιr wire n sãsιrɛ kho kpɛɛrɛ yaa, ga-n sãsa?
42014004	Dι wι pιr pɔɔpɔɔ. Dι Jeju fʋ khodaarιle a kpɛɛ ɔɔ kho sa sιιraa dι bir kɔ̃.
42014005	Agιpι Jeju bule wi: Ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil nɛrɛra ado ɔɔ bi ji birera, agιbo ɔɔ nake gι, a na tii dapaara khə̃khə̃ hιιr wirəə?
42014006	Dι wa kɔɔ puno a na birsee gelela bã.
42014007	Agιpι a sor wιrɛraakɛ wι kɔɔ wenι dιkorra sokpa bιɛl, gιdonι a yιrɛ mɔ̃kɛ wι-n phiirni ƴɛ kʋʋl too pa. Dɩ a so warɛ:
42014008	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil we fɩnɩ dɩkorra dɩ fɩ jal, fa-n gba too paar ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ afɩ dɩbara ga. Agakpaana tibil kpɩɩkɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ fɩ hale, kɛ wɩ wenɩ dakha;
42014009	dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛra kɔɔ wɛ nɩnɩ fɛʋ na pɔr na so far: Hana ʋrɛ too paarɩkɛra. Le yicuru na fʋ fɩ mɔ̃kɛ fa-n birni pɩpɩɩ too paarra.
42014010	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ we fɩnɩ dɩkorra dɩ fɩ jal, tɔɔ pɩpɩɩ too paarra, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ wɛ fɩnɩ na lonɩ a na so farɛ: Ɩ̃ kuun, ɩrɛ a ɩna tɔɔ kɛkɛ ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ. Le ga do far cʋrɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ fɩ hananɩ kha dɩko kho paar.
42014011	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n kanɩ ire wa wuruure, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n wuroni dɩbara, ɔr wa ɩɩr.
42014012	Dɩ Jeju so ʋrɛraakɛ kɔɔ wɩɛnɩ dakha ayɩ: Dabɔɔkɛ fɩ-n wenɩ tɩbɩla nɩ khɔ kha dɩkor, a ʋlkhɔɔ gɩ, a dɩtɩnɔ gɩ, fa-n we afɩ kuunsɔ, agɩbo afɩ õkuunsɔ, agɩbo afɩ toosɔ, agɩbo afɩ cɔ khu lẽledarasɔa'. Gɩdonɩ agakpaana wa we fer dakha wer, gɩ ho wɩ lɩmɩ fɛr.
42014013	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ-n wenɩ tɩbɩla dɩkorra, wɛ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ bɔdara, na tãdara, na nɛ kʋɛdarasɔ, na yarasɔ.
42014014	Dɩ ga da farɛ gɩdonɩ wa hana thɩ̃ɛ a na lɩmɩ fa', sɩ Thãgba gɩɩkɛ na lɩma fɩnɩ wireekɛ tɩɩ sara na ɩɩrnɩ na the khirera.
42014015	Dɩ tibil bɩɛl wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ tɔɔnɩ dɩko kho paarɩle, ɔbɔɔkɛ a nɩɛnɩ thɩmɩɩrɩle pɩ, a sor Jejura: Ga dar ʋrɛraakɛ na khɔnɩ dɩkor Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
42014016	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ cʋʋ fɛtɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ a wena tɩbɩla jɔɔ.
42014017	A dɩko kho bɔɔ dã, a thʋɔn ɔɔ thɔ̃daar a jala a wɛ wɩrɛɛkɛra a kɔɔ wenɩ wɩ pɔ, gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ.
42014018	Sɩ wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl mar dɩ wa-n ther thɩ̃ɛsɔ dɩɩdɩɩ: Cacadaar sʋʋraarɛ: Mɩ kɔɔ ther lɛ phaa dɩɩ teena ɩ̃ jala hɩnɛ. Mɩ-n bɩɛl fɛr ma 'lɛ na pɔa'.
42014019	Dɩ ʋ yɩ: Mɩ kɔɔ ther nakena yʋɔr dɩ ma-n jal ɩ̃ dona wɩ thɔma ɩ̃ hɩɩn. Mɩ-n bɩɛl fɛr ma 'lɛ na pɔa'.
42014020	Dɩ ʋ so wo: Mɩ her khɛr he phaa, dɩ gɛr gɩ ma 'lɛ na pɔa'.
42014021	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ thɔ̃daarɩle kɔɔ birni dã cʋɔr, a mɩɩrɛ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ thɩ̃ therresɔɔlera fɛʋ. Dɩ nĩkhii fʋ cɔdaar kuun, dɩ so ɔɔ thɔ̃daarra ayɩ: Birə jala khə̃khə̃khə̃ a lona dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ƴatɔɔ na hʋ kɔ̃tɩnana, a kpa bɔdarasɔ, na tãdarasɔ, na yarasɔ, na nɛ kʋɛdarasɔ a ɛna kɛ.
42014022	Dɩ thɔ̃daarɩle sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, gɩrɛɛkɛra fɩ kɔɔ sonɩ mɩ cʋʋrɛ pɩ, sɩ too paar bo sɩrakɛ wo 'lo.
42014023	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn so ɔɔ thɔ̃daarra: Birə gba hʋɛsɔ na jala na hʋ sɔ̃sʋ̃ɔsɔ, a yɩrana tɩbɩla wɩ lõ wɩ hi ɩ̃ cɔ phi.
42014024	Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ, tibil bɩɛl wɩrɛraakɛ mɩ kɔɔ wenɩ na 'lɛ ɩ̃ dɩkora bã.
42014025	Tibil jɔjʋɔ n kɔɔ kpar Jejura, dɩ kɛr a so war:
42014026	A tibil na ɩ̃ mɛrɛra sɩ aa-n laar ɔɔ tha', na ɔɔ na', na ɔɔ khɛra', na ɔɔ bɩsãsɔa', na ɔɔ õkonasɔa', na ɔɔ õkhɛrsɔa', na ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ yə', a na puno na do ɩ̃ kpãkpãadaara'.
42014027	Dɩ ntɛɛkɛ na-n heenenɩ ɔɔ kʋkʋ thɩr da-n kpana mara', a na puno na do ɩ̃ kpãkpãadaara'.
42014028	Gɩdonɩ ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil nɛrɛra ado a ƴaal a mɩ cɔ gbãa, ga do a na toore ɓo a ther gɩrɛɛkɛ a na kʋɛnɩ a hɩɩn, ado a hananɛ gɩrɛ na dananaa?
42014029	A mɛ̃ gaa, ɔbɔɔkɛ a kpɛɛnɩ go kʋʋ pɩ sɩ aa puno pa', wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na yɩɛnɩ wa-n maanʋʋnɛ wa-n sonaa wɩ yɩ aa:
42014030	Hɩnɛ, kuunikɛ kɔɔ fʋrɛ da-n mɩ cɔ gbãa, sɩ aa puno kpoora'.
42014031	Dɩ agɩbo wo, ʋmɔ̃ɔ fãgadaar na-n jala a ke kʋʋr na ʋ̃ fãgadaar, sɩɩ do aa kɔɔ too ɓo a gʋʋr a hɩɩn, ado a na punone na kona gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr a na caan ole hananɩ kona gbɩlanɩ kpelẽ da-n pɔnanaa ga?
42014032	Ado a na punoə', mee ɔbɔɔkɛ wa fãgadaarɩle hanɩnakɛ ƴɔɔ, ƴɛƴɛa a na thɔ̃ wɩ caanɛ ƴɛgaa?
42014033	Mɛ̃ gɩ dakha, ntɛɛkɛ na-n bɔnɩ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a hɩna', a na puno na do ɩ̃ kpãkpãadaara'.
42014034	Thɩ̃ bʋɔ laan do, sɩ a laan bir dasɩ a mɩla bã, mɔ̃ wa fʋ sɩ na cʋʋ dɩ a bir na hana mɩlalɛ?
42014035	Ga taa thɩɩ bʋɔa', dɩ ga do beethɩn woa'. Khuirə wa dʋna na faa. Ntɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu dɩ nɩna, dɔ a na-n pɛ nũu.
42015001	Dɩ war gbadara na sopugodara fɛʋ kɔɔ tɔr wɔrɔ̃ Jeju, dɩ wa-n pɩɛ nũu.
42015002	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na-n hũhuun kha dɩ wa-n sona aa: Kuunikɛ a-n teere sopugodara kpakpaalɛ dɩ wa-n kho kha dɩkor.
42015003	Dɩ Jeju so war sokpaakɛ:
42015004	Ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil nɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn na hana banaa tamaa dɩ bɩɛl na bu, sɩɩ do aa faa tamaa phe bireele sɛnɩ khʋʋl paar, sa jal a ƴaal bιɛlιle bonι phaphapha a yιa'.
42015005	Mee a a yιι pι, a na gbaarɛ na daʋ a na pɛ ɔɔ nyɔ̃ gbɛgbɛlla.
42015006	A a dã cʋɔr, a na wer ɔɔ kuunsɔ na ɔɔ cɔ khudarasɔ na so war nayι: Nι dɔ sa-n kãka kha, gιdonι mι bire yι ɩ̃ banaakɛra kɔɔ bonι.
42015007	Mɩ so narɛ, thale daʋ na ha Thãgbaa dʋɔ sopugodaar bιɛlι ha debira, a na jɔ tιɩ sara tamaa phe bireekɛ na-n ƴaalɛnɩ ha debira'.
42015008	Dɩ agɩbo, ʋmɔ̃ɔ khɛr na hana sẽkãsɩ yʋɔr dɩ bɩɛl na bu, sɩɩ do aa pɛ lãphã sa kpabɩ cʋɔr a jɩɩ ƴaal phaphapha a yɩ ga?
42015009	Mee a a yɩ gɩ, a na wer ɔɔ kuunsɔ na ɔɔ cɔ khudarasɔ wɩ pɔ a so war ayɩ: Nɩ dɔ sa-n kãka kha, gɩdonɩ mɩ bire yɩ sẽkãsɩɩkɛ kɔɔ bo mɩnɩ.
42015010	Mɩ so narɛ, thale daʋ na ha Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn sopugodaar bɩɛllaakɛ n debanɩ haar.
42015011	Dι Jeju so war wo ayι: Kũu bιɛl gι, a hana bikona yenyɔ.
42015012	Dι bikũu diine so ɔɔ thιra: Ɩ̃ thι, ha mι gιrɛ na dɔnι ɩ̃da. Dι ɔɔ thι tιnɛ wι ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔ wɛr yenyɔra fɛʋ.
42015013	Ga pʋɔra' sι bikũu diine ιιr a khιι ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔ fɛʋ, a jalna dι kpιιra ƴɔɔ fĩi. Le a jãjalã ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔra khaarkhaar cʋʋrɛra.
42015014	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ pι, kɔmɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι lʋʋn dιιraalera, dι le bʋɔ ma dι a-n fʋʋ.
42015015	Dι ιιr jal tibil bιɛlla dιιraale a gba nι thɔma, dι gbaa pɛ ɔɔ lɔɔ a na-n khɛ nι dabulo sιthɔsɔ.
42015016	Dι a kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar, ιna-n khɔra dιkɔɔkɛ dabulo sιthɔsɔ n khonι, sι tibil na-n haa ga.
42015017	Le fιlɛ n ιnaa dιphã, dι so ɔɔbara: Ɩ̃ thιι cɔ thɔ̃dara yemɔ̃ haanle gιrɛ, kɛ n khɔnι dιkɔ dι wι hi sa sι, sι me wer, kɔmɛr na-n lιɛr mι kɛkɛ.
42015018	Ma ιιrɛ a na bir ɩ̃ thιι pa na sʋʋraa nayι: Ɩ̃ thι, mι cʋʋrɛ sopugo Thãgbara na fɛrɛra.
42015019	Ma teena dι wa we mι afι bikũu bιnɔ 'lo bã, sι gba mι ɩ̃ ho afι thɔ̃daar bιɛl.
42015020	Dι le a ιιr da-n bir ɔɔ thιra. Sι dabɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ hanι ƴɔɔ fĩi, ɔɔ thι yιιrɛ dι bʋɔ fʋʋ, dι ca caan a fʋʋ a pal.
42015021	Dι bikuun sʋʋraa: Ɩ̃ thι, mι cʋʋrɛ sopugo Thãgbara na fɛrɛra, ma teena dι wa we mι afι bikũu bιnɔ 'lo bã.
42015022	Dι thιrɛ sor ɔɔ thɔ̃darara: Nι gba kẽkẽ gbãakɛ ɓɔnanι a jɔ kẽkena fɛʋ, a ɛna kɔrɔ a tʋɔnɛɛ, a tɔnaa nyɛ̃bi tʋʋ a tʋɔnɛɛ nɛfaa.
42015023	Nι fɔ naɓol khʋ̃ɔ a ɛna kɔ,
42015024	sɩ kho sa-n kãkana, gιdonι ɩ̃ bikuunikɛ a kɔɔ khire sι a bire a hana yire. A kɔɔ bure sι sι yιιrɛ. Dι wι mar dι wa-n kãka.
42015025	Sι bikũu kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ har lɔɔ. Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ thenι lɔɔ da-n ɩ̃ a thɔɔ cɔ nʋɔ, a nιɛrɛ bιna dι wa-n sa.
42015026	Dι a wer thɔ̃daar bιɛl a bulee thɩ̃ doo n cʋɛnι thale.
42015027	Dι thɔ̃daarde sʋʋraa: Afι õkuun birə ɩ̃, dι gιdonι afι thι bire yιι na tomι kheu, gɛr gɩ dɩ kʋʋ naɓol khʋ̃ɔ.
42015028	Dι nĩkhii fʋrɛ bikũu kɔ̃tιn dι bo cɔ lʋʋn. Dι ɔɔ thι the a phʋʋrʋʋ a lona.
42015029	Dι le a so ɔɔ thιra: Hιnɛ, yɛna jɔrɛ ka mι do fιnι thɔma, dι ma kɔɔ nʋʋr nũu afɩ jɔfʋ bɩɛlla yuuraka', sɩ fa kɔɔ ha mɩnakɛ bʋ̃bir ɩ̃ ɓolana ɩ̃ kuunsɔ babɩɛla'.
42015030	Sɩ afɩ bikuunikɛ ɩnanɩ gɩrɛ, ʋrɛɛkɛ kanɩ kɔɔ jãjalã afɩ thɩ̃sɔ bɔdɛlasɔra, ɔr fɩ ka kʋ naɓol khʋ̃ɔ.
42015031	Dɩ ɔɔ thɩ sʋʋraa: Fɛr ɩ̃ bɩsã, fɩ har kha na mɛrɛ wire fɛʋ, dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ hananɩ afɩda gɩ do.
42015032	Sɩ gɩ teenanɛ sɩ ɓola a na kãkanɛna, gɩdonɩ afɩ õkuunikɛ a kɔɔ khire, sɩ a bire a hana yire, dɩ dakha a kɔɔ bure, sɩ sɩ bire yɩɩ.
42016001	Dɩ Jeju sor dakha ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Lẽle kuun gɩ, a kɔɔ hale a hana thɩ̃ hɩɩndaar bɩɛl, dɩ wɩ pɔ a sʋʋraa mɔ̃ ɔɔ thɩ̃ hɩɩndaarra n kʋɛnɩ ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔ.
42016002	Dɩ lẽle kuunile wɩɩrɛ a bulee: Anye ha gɩrɛ mɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ fɛrɛra? Thera thɩ̃ɛsɔ a nɛna mɩ ɩ̃ hɩɩn, gɩdonɩ fa puno a na do ɩ̃ thɩ̃ hɩɩndaar bã.
42016003	Dɩ thɩ̃ hɩɩndaarɩle so ɔɔ bara: Anye ma cʋʋ ya fɛ? Gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na faa mɛr. Ɩ̃ kʋʋl yaa? Sɩ ma hana fãga woa'. Ma-n bɩɛl yaa? Sɩ yicuru na fʋ mɛr.
42016004	Mɩ jɩrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ma cʋʋnɩ dɩphã, dɩ tɩbɩla na tee mɩ awɩ cɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ na faa mɩnɩ.
42016005	Dɩ le a we wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ pemanɩ thɩ̃ɛ ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩna bɩɛlbɩɛl fɛʋ, a bule cacadaar: Yemɔ̃ fɩ hana ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ helu?
42016006	Dɩ birsee: Balãga niin tamaa gɩ. Dɩ thɩ̃ hɩɩndaar sʋʋraa: Gba afɩ sɛbɛ a tɔɔ khə̃khə̃, a kherene kpalanyɔ yʋɔr.
42016007	Agɩpɩ dɩ bule ʋ̃ wo ayɩ: Sɩ fɛrɛ yemɔ̃ afɩ hel ha? Dɩ birsee: Jʋ kpona tamaa gɩ. Dɩ sʋʋraa: Gba afɩ sɛbɛ a kherene kpalanã.
42016008	Dɩ kɔ̃tɩn khɩɩrɛ bubur thɩ̃ hɩɩndaarɩle, mɔ̃ a hananɩ kpɩɛrɛ gbãʋ thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra. Gɩdonɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ bɩsãsɔ n kpɩɛrɛ gbãʋ na awɩ hohosɔ a jɔ dahɩrɛɛ bɩsãsɔ.
42016009	Sɩ mɛrɛ mɩ so narɛ: Nɩ gba lẽle thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ na sarana' a kurona kuune, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ga pɩnɩ, wa tee ner dɩ na lõ khorr waara.
42016010	Tibilikɛ dʋɔnnɩ sobɔ cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ biisɔra, mɛna a na do sobɔ cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩnasɔra dakha. Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ bubur cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ biisɔra, mɛna a na do bubur cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩnasɔra dakha.
42016011	Ado mɛ̃ gɩ, ado na kɔɔ do sobɔ cʋʋdara lẽle thɩ̃ɛsɔraakɛ na saranaa ga, amɛ na pɛ nar nɩ dɔ sobɔ lẽle thɩ̃ hɩɩndara?
42016012	Dɩ ado na kɔɔ do sobɔ cʋʋdara gɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ tibil kpɩɩda ga, amɛ na hana nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ anɩda?
42016013	Thɔ̃daar na hale a na puno na do thɔma kɔ̃tɩna yenyɔra ga, foo a na laarɛ bɩɛl sɩ a na na bɩɛl, agɩbo a na mar kha na bɩɛl sɩ a hɛbɩ bɩɛl. Na puno na do thɔma Thãgbara nakha lẽle thɩ̃a'.
42016014	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔɔkɛ dʋɔnnɩ war nadara kɔɔ hale dɩ wa-n pɛ thɩmɩaalera fɛʋ nũu, dɩ wɩ-n maanɛ Jejura.
42016015	Dɩ so war: Nɛrɛ, nɛr dʋɔn tɩbɩlaakɛ n cʋɛnɩ dɩ nɩ ho fɩl sardara tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra, sɩ Thãgba jɩrɛ anɩ hasɔ. Gɩdonɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ tɩbɩla n hɩɩnnɩ dɩɩ do thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, gɛr dʋɔn kpɔ̃kpɔrɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra.
42016016	A dana Jã Batɩsɩtɩɩ bɔɔ, jɔfʋ na Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ haanle. Dɩ a fʋna ɔbɔɔlera, gɛr wɩ-n mɩɩrɔ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩda, dɩ tɩbɩla bɩɛlbɩɛl fɛʋ n pɛrɛ fãga ɩnɩ-n lona Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
42016017	Sɩ thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩ pho ka yɔɔrɛ a ka jɔ dɩkhaa thɩ̃ bu bɩɛl fɩɩʋ jɔfʋra faa.
42016018	A tibil faa ɔɔ khɛr sa bir a he khɛ kpɩɩ, khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaal sopugo a cʋʋ. Dɩ tibilikɛ na gbaannɩ khɛrɩkɛ ɔɔ ko faanɩ, khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaal sopugo a cʋʋ.
42016019	Lẽle kũu bιɛl gι, a kɔɔ hale dι to gbιlã kẽkena, dι wire fɛʋ a-n kãka da-n phιphιlana.
42016020	Dι bɔdaar kuun hale dakha dι wa-n wιι Lajaar, dι nɔra teguu tomιr koo da-n phιna lẽle kuuni lõfonɔra.
42016021	Dι a kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar ιna-n khɔ dιkorιkɛ n jaalɛnι lẽle kuuni dιko kho pa. Dι benaa thɛthɛ n pʋɔnnakɛ dι wa-n dɛlɛ̃ ɔɔ nɔrsɔra.
42016022	Dι bɔdaar kuunilera khire, dι Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ gbaa a jalna Abιrahamι pa. Dι lẽle kuun dakha ɩ̃ a khi dι wι dʋʋ.
42016023	Dɩ le khĩdi dʋɔ mɔ̃kɛ a-n yɩnɩ bɔ gaarɛ jɔɔ, a gbaar da-n hɩɩn a 'laa yɩ Abɩraham ƴɔɔ fĩi, dɩ Lajaar too ɔɔ kal ƴɔɔ.
42016024	Dɩ le a hulẽ ayɩ: Ɩ̃ thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abɩraham, jɛ mɩ bʋɔrarakɛ sa thɔna Lajaar a ɓɛ nyʋɔn na ɔɔ nyɛ̃bi a ɩna a ɩɛna mɩ delẽbire, gɩdonɩ mɩ-n gaarɛ bʋɔ ka dɔlɩnanɛnaakɛ.
42016025	Sɩ Abɩraham birsee: Ɩ̃ bɩsã, jɛna fɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr bɔɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ kɔɔ hanɩle thɩɩra, sɩ dɩ dakha Lajaar kɔɔ 'lɛ puure. Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ a hakɛ a faa haar, sɩ fɛrɛ dɩ fa-n gaar.
42016026	Sɩ ga dorakɛ gele koo gɩ dɩbara woa', sɩ kõkor pɛ hulõo hakɛ sɛrɛ na nɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ hanɩkɛ sa ƴaal wɩ seer le anɩ pa, wa punoə'. Dι dakha, wιrɛɛkɛ hana fιnι le sa ƴaal wι seer kɛ asι pa, wa punoə'.
42016027	Dι lẽle kuun sʋʋraa: Dι a mɛ̃ gι, mι-n bιɛl fɛr thιrɛ dι fa thɔ̃ Lajaar ɩ̃ thιι cɔ, gιdonι mι hananɛ õkona yemɔι,
42016028	a jala a kpãkpaanɛ war. Ado mɛ̃ gaa, wɛr dakha wa ιnɛ 'wãga paarιkɛra.
42016029	Dι Abιraham birsee: Wι hananɛ sɛbɛsɔɔkɛ Mʋɩjɩ na Thãgbaa bobonasɔ kɔɔ kherenι. Dɔ wι pɛ wele nũu.
42016030	Dι lẽle kuun bir birsee: Kpeehe ɩ̃ thι kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abιraham, a kĩdidaar bιɛl jala a yι wι wa debire haar.
42016031	Dι Abιraham sʋʋraa: A wa pɛ Mʋιjι na Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔda nũə', sι dι khĩdidaar bɩɛl ɩɩrrakɛ a the khirera, ga cʋʋ wɩ dɩ wa pɛr haara'.
42017001	Jeju sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Ka paar na hale sɩ gɩ do nɛ baradaasɔ na halaa ga, sɩ ga puure ʋrɛraakɛ n cʋɛ gɩnɩ dɩ ga-n hale.
42017002	A wɩ gba nã kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ tə̃ə, a li tibilləəle fʋɔrɔ sa dʋnaa lanyʋɔnɔ, ga baar gɩrɛɛkɛ a na kanɩ na cʋʋ bɩsã biikɛra bɩɛl dɩ na bara.
42017003	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ. Ado afɩ omi cʋʋrɛ sopugo, phaanɛɛ, dɩ ado a debi haar faa hanaa.
42017004	Dɩ adorakɛ a cʋʋ fɩ puure wi bɩɛl nyɛ̃be makonyɔ, sa bir pɔ far nyɛ̃be makonyɔra a so far ayɩ, ɩnɩ debire haar, dɔ fɩ faa fɩ haa.
42017005	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔna so Kɔ̃tɩnna: Dɛba sar ha pɛrɛ.
42017006	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn birse wi: Ado nɩ kɔɔ hananɛna ha pɛrɛ dɩɩ ho seneve bireekɛ n hanɩ fɩɩʋ, na punone na sona thɩrʋraakɛ nayɩ: Ǝlə a jala thera lanyɔ̃ bɩnɔ dɩbara, dɩ a na nɩ nɛr nũu.
42017007	Amɛ nɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn na hana thɔ̃daar a na-n kʋʋlʋʋ, agɩbo a na-n khɩɩ nʋma, a a the lɔɔ na ɩ̃ gɩ do a sʋʋraarɛ waa ayɩ, a ɩna kɔrɔ a tɔɔ khɔ dɩkor?
42017008	Ga do a na ka na sʋʋraarɛ nayɩ: Cʋɛ mɩ dɩkor, sa gbɛbɩrɛ ɩ̃ dɩko thɩɩn gbɛbɩrɩ. A mɩ kho dɩphã a yɔna a pɩ, fɩ kho fer fɩ yɔna gaa?
42017009	A na fʋɔrɛ ɔɔ thɔ̃daar, gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ pɩɛraanɩ ya?
42017010	Mɛ̃ gɩ ha na nɛrɛ dakha. Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ cʋʋnɩ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wι pɛ narnι pɩ, nɩ sɔ ayɛwɔɔ: Mɔlɔ thɔ̃ dona ha sɩ, dɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ teananɩ sɩ cʋɛ sɩ cʋʋ.
42017011	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju hanɩ hʋɛra da-n jal Jerujalɛm, a kɔɔ kanaɛ hʋɛɛkɛ hanɩ Samarɩ na Galile thɩ̃thɩɩn.
42017012	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ a pɔnɩ da-n lõ dɩ bɩɛlla, gbulo yʋɔr gbaar dɩ wa-n caanʋʋna sa jɩɩl ƴɔɔ gbe;
42017013	sɩ wa-n hulẽ: Jeju Dɩɩrdaar, jɛ sɩ bʋɔra.
42017014	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju y wɩnɩ a so warɛ: Nɩ jala nɛna Thãgbaa bonɩ jidara mɔ̃ nɩ hanɩ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ gbanɩ hʋɛ dɩ wa-n jal, awɩ gbuul pɩ warɛ hʋɛrara.
42017015	Sɩ bɩɛl wɛrra ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ yɩɛnɩ dɩ ɔɔ gbuul pɩrɛ, a kɛrrɛ bir dapaara da-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i na nɔ kheu.
42017016	Dɩ a jire Jejuu ƴɛra a sumo da-n fʋɔrʋʋ; Samarɩdaar bɩɛl gɩ.
42017017	Dɩ Jeju so: Ga do tɩbɩla yʋɔr gbuule kɔɔ pɩrɔaa? Sɩ yʋɔr phebireekɛ sɛnɩ ka wɩ ha?
42017018	Agado kpakpalɩle ga, tibil bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ hale a bir a dʋbɩ Thãgbaa iə'.
42017019	Agɩpɩ dɩ sʋʋraa: Ɩrɛ birə kɔna, afɩ ha pɛ taa fɩ.
42017020	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ bule Jeju wɩ jɩ bɔɔkɛ Thãgba na gbani fãga, dɩ Jeju birse wi: Thãgbaa fãgadaar do na ɩ̃ gɩ do tibil yɩɛra'.
42017021	Dɩ wa puno na so nayɩ: Nɩ hɩnɛ kɩɛr gɩ, agɩbo pal ga, gɩdom Thãgbaa fãgadaar do anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn gɩ ha.
42017022	Dɩ a sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara wo: Bɔ bɩɛl na daan dɩ na ƴaal mɛr tibili Bikuuni wi n phana, sɩ na yɩ ga.
42017023	Wa so narɛ nayι: Nι hιnɛ kιɛr a ha, agιbo pal a ha. Na-n jala', dι na-n ca na kpa wara'.
42017024	Gιdonι mɔ̃kɛ thãgba n lenι dɔɔ ʋ̃ gɛllɔ dιι hιrɛ a carbara a ka thʋ ʋ̃ gɛl, mɛ̃ mɛr tibili Bikuun na ha ɩ̃ wirə.
42017025	Sι gι teenanɛ ɩ̃ kɔɔ gaar bʋɔ ɓo nĩdaraakɛ n bo mι.
42017026	Gιrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananι Noee bɔɔ, oti ga dã tibili Bikuuni bɔɔ dakha.
42017027	Tιbιla n kɔɔ khor dιkɔ dι wa-n yɔna, dι wa-n hena kha dι wa-n 'laana awι bisɔ herra phaphapha dιι ba dana Noee bato lõ wi waa dιphã, dι nyʋɔn kɔɔ phã a gbʋma wι dι wι khiir fɛʋ.
42017028	Ga har mɔ̃kɛ gι kɔɔ hanι Lɔtιι bɔɔ. Wι-n kɔɔ khor dιkɔ dι wa-n yɔna, dι wa-n thena thɩ̃ɛsɔ dι wa-n dolona thɩ̃ɛ, dι wa-n diirnə, dι wa-n mιna cɔna.
42017029	Sι wireekɛ Lɔtι kɔɔ thenι Sɔdɔm, gɛr dɔɔ na girbi kɔɔ the ƴũ a gbũ a thii wi fɛʋ.
42017030	Mɛ̃ ga ha wireraakɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun na nιnanι ɩ̃bara.
42017031	Dawiilera, ʋrɛɛkɛ na hanι nãsʋrɔ sι dι ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔ ha cɔ bιnɔ, a na gbũ na gba bã, dι ʋrɛɛkɛ dakha na hanι lɔɔ, a na kɛr na hir bã.
42017032	Na-n jɛna Lɔtɩι khɛrɩda.
42017033	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩna-n tɛba ɩnɩ yi, ga ka na buurəəre, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛɛ yi kanɩ bu, ɔr na ka na 'lɛ.
42017034	Mɩ so narɛ, ga dɩtɩnɔɔlera tɩbɩla yenyɔ na hale phɩ̃ pa bɩɛl, Thãgba na gbaar bɩɛl sɩ na faa bɩɛl.
42017035	Dɩ khɛra yenyɔɔkɛ na hanɩ kha jʋ nã paar, Thãgba na gbaar bɩɛl sɩ na faa bɩɛl.
42017036	[Kona yenyɔ na hale lɛ bɩɛlla, Thãgba na gbaar bɩɛl sɩ na faa bɩɛl.]
42017037	Dɩ kpãkpãadara bulee: Kɔ̃tɩn, kana gɩrɛɛkɛra na dã? Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Kãkɛ thɩ̃ khire hanɩ, le dũusɔ na caan kha.
42018001	Dɩ Jeju so war sokpa bɩɛl, a nɩna wɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ teenanɩ wa-n bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba wire fɛʋ sɩ wa-n vɔa', ayɩ:
42018002	So kɩɩldaar bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hale dɩ bɩɛlla. Aa-n ma Thãgba ga, aa-n therna tibil dakha ga.
42018003	Dɩ khikhɛr bɩɛl kɔɔ hale dɩɩraalera dakha, kɛ n pʋɔnnɩ ɔɔ pa da-n sʋʋraa: Wɛ ɩ̃ sodaar a ɩ̃ fɩ gʋʋr sɩ sor.
42018004	A a pɔ dɩ so kɩɩldaarɩle n bo, a a pɔ dɩ bo, sɩ agɩpɩ a bire so ɔɔbara: Sobɔr gɩ wer, ma-n ma Thãgba ga, dɩ tibil gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ therna ga.
42018005	Sɩ gɩdonɩ khikhɛrʋʋkɛra n vɔɔ mɛr thakɛ, ma gʋʋrɛ ɔɔdara, a mɛ̃ gaa a na ɩnɛ a na-n vɔɔ mɩ ƴɛrr.
42018006	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn so: Nɩ nɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ gõgolõ so kɩɩldaar kɔɔ sonɩ pal;
42018007	sɩ Thãgba a na ka na nɩna wɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ phiirni ɔɔ fɩl sar, kɛ n hulenenaanɩ dɩwɩlʋ na dɩtɩnɔ fɛʋaa? A na pʋɔrɛ sa a nɩna wɩ ya?
42018008	Mɩ so narɛ a na nɩna wɛr dapaara ɔɔ fɩl sar. Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun na birni na ɩ̃, ma yɩrɛ ha pɛrɛ thɩɩra bɛ?
42018009	Jeju sor sokpa bɩɛl wo wɩrɛraakɛ n kpɩɛrɛnɩ ɩnɩ dor fɩl sardara, sɩ dɩ wa-n beesi ʋkhasɔ, a sor ayɩ:
42018010	Tɩbɩla yenyɔ wɛ, dɩ wa-n jal Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna wɩ bɩɛl Thãgba. Bɩɛl do jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar, sɩ bɩɛl do war gbadaar.
42018011	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar jɩɩl ƴũ jɩɩlɔ da-n bɩɛl ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ dɩbara thakɛ: Ɩ̃ Thãgba, mɩ-n fʋɔr fɛr gɩrɛraakɛ ma honanɩ tibil ɩkhasɔa', kɛ dɔnɩ tɩɩ tagɩrɩdara', agɩbo wɩrɛ na saranaa ga, dɩ khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaaldara gɩ woa', dɩ war gbadaarɩkɛ gɩrakɛ woa'.
42018012	Mɩ-n lire nʋɔ balanyɔ wire makonyɔra, mɩ-n 'laarɛ dakha bɩɛl yʋɔr thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋraakɛ mɩ n 'lɛnι.
42018013	Sι war gbadaarιle jιιlɛ ƴɔɔ gbe, aa 'la na hɩɩn ƴũə' sa gʋɛ ƴιɛ thιιra a so: Pha Thãgba, jɛ mɛr sopugodaarɩkɛ bʋɔra.
42018014	Mɩ so narɛ, tibililera ka fire kɔna so hɛllɛ, sɩ ole wer, kpei. Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n kanɩ ire, wa wuruure, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n wuroni dɩbara, ɔr wa ɩɩr.
42018015	Dɩ tɩbɩla kɔɔ gbaar awɩ bisɔ a pɔna Jejura a dɛɛnɛ war nyɛ̃ɛ, sɩ mɔ̃ kpãkpãadara yɩnɩ gelela, wɩ kɔɔ phaanɛ wɩrɛ pɔna wɩnɩ.
42018016	Dɩ Jeju we wɩ wɩ pɔna wɩ, sɩ a sor: Nɩ dɔ bɩsana na-n ɩ̃ mar na-n pɩɛr wa', gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ hɔnɩ bɩsana, wɛr Thãgbaa fãgadaar do mana.
42018017	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n tuonni Thãgbaa fãgadaar do bɩsanaa khaaka', a na puno na lono kpɩɩraka'.
42018018	Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ bule Jeju thakɛ ayɩ: Dɩɩrdaar bʋɔ, anye ma cʋʋ na 'lɛ yire khorr?
42018019	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fɩ we mɩ dabʋɔ? Tɩɩ bʋɔ na hala', Thãgba dɩbara bʋɔnɔ.
42018020	Fɩ jɩrɛ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ: “Fa-n hana khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n hana kũu kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n kʋ tibilə', fa-n yuə', fa-n sõso pɛ tibilə', na cɔ afɩ thɩ na afɩ nɩ.”
42018021	Dɩ kuunile birsee: Mɩ kɔɔ mãa nɩ ga jɔfʋraale fɛʋ nũu kɛkɛkɛ ɩ̃ daɓol dĩi bɔɔ.
42018022	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ gele a sʋʋraarɛ: Thɩ̃ bɩɛl ɓɔr fɛr wo. Jala dolone thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ fɩ hananɩ a hana bɔdara, dɩ mɛ̃ fa 'lɛ lẽle thɩ̃ɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, agɩpɩ fɩ ɩ̃ fa-n kpa mar.
42018023	Ɔbɔɔkɛ kuunile nɩɛnɩ gele a gbure ƴɩɛ, gɩdonɩ lẽledaar gɩ na sobɔr.
42018024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju yɩɩnɩ dɩ gbu ƴɩɛ a sor: Thãgba fãgadaar dɩ lʋʋn khɩɩrɛ waa gel wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ lɛ̃lɛ.
42018025	Gɩdonɩ nyɔɔmɛɛ lõokɛ a na lonɩ mɩsɩmɩ kaar ka yɔɔrɛ jɔ lẽlee Thãgba fãgadaar dɩ lõ.
42018026	Dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ so: Dɩ a mɛ̃ gɩ, amɛ na punone na 'lɛ taarɛ?
42018027	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Gɩrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ thɩ̃ punonaa tɩbɩlala ga, gɛr Thãgba n ka puno.
42018028	Dɩ Pɩɛr so: Hɩnɛ, sɛrɛ sɩ faarɛ asɩ thɩ̃sɔ fɛʋ sɩ sa-n kpa far.
42018029	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, tibil na faa ɔɔ cɔ, a ɔɔ khɛr gɩ, a ɔɔ õkuunsɔ wɛ, a ɔɔ thɩ gɩ, a ɔɔ nɩ gɩ, a ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ wɛ, gɩ do Thãgbaa fãgadaar do dɔ nɔɔ,
42018030	sɩɩ do aa 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛ dɩɩ jɔ gɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ faanaa ga, dɩ bɔɔkɛ na ɩnanɩ dakha a na 'lɛr yire khorr.
42018031	Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ kpar yʋɔr yenyɔ dι wι ha kha, dι so war: Nι hɩnɛ Jerujalɛm sι-n jal gιrɛ, dι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ kherenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra mɛr tibili Bikuunna na daan.
42018032	Gιdonι wa fʋ mɛr na ha ca kpala, dι wa mãa mɛr a na kpoona mar, wι cιιrna nyɔ̃thɩ̃ι wa-n pɛ mar.
42018033	A wι ciil mi na khasa pι, wa kʋ mɛr. Sι wire yẽther wirera ma ιιrɛ na the khirera.
42018034	Sι kpãkpãadara na kɔɔ jι gar thɩ̃ bιɛllaka'. Thιmιι caale kɔɔ ker warɛ, wa jι gι kιrʋa'.
42018035	Mɔ̃kɛ Jeju n wɔrɔnι Jeriko, yaar bιɛl gι, a kɔɔ hale a too hʋ nʋɔra da-n bιɛl thɩ̃ɛ.
42018036	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a nιɛnι tibil jɔ dι wa-n ka, a bulele a jι kιrʋ.
42018037	Dι wι sʋʋraa: Najarɛtι Jeju n ka.
42018038	Dι hulẽ: Jeju, Davιdιι Bikuun, jɛ mι bʋɔra.
42018039	Dι wιrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hanι ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ, wι manaanɛ ayι a pιra, sι a ka jιɛ bir hulẽ wo: Davιdιι Bikuun, jɛ mι bʋɔra.
42018040	Dι Jeju jιιl sa yι wι kpaa pɔna. Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a danι, Jeju buleele:
42018041	Anye fι-n ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋɛ far? Dι birsee: Kɔ̃tιn, cʋɛ mι ma-n yɩ.
42018042	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dι khɛra, afι ha pɛ taa fι.
42018043	Dι dapaara ɔɔ yi khɛr da-n yι, a kpa Jejura da-n dʋbιna Thãgbaa i. Ɔbɔɔkɛ tιbιla fɛʋ yιnι gelela wι khιιrɛ Thãgba.
42019001	Dι Jeju lʋʋn Jeriko a kpãsɛ da-n jal.
42019002	Dɩ hɩnɛ, lẽle kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a hale dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Jase, war gbadaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃ a do.
42019003	Dɩ a ƴaalɛ a jɩ ntɛɛkɛ Jeju donɩ, sɩ aa puno na yɩɩ tibil jɔraala', gɩdonɩ a gburore.
42019004	Dɩ a car jal ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ a jʋʋn thɩrʋra a yɩ Jeju, gɩdonɩ le a teena a kana.
42019005	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju danɩ paarɩlera, a gbaar hɩɩn ƴũ sa wɩɩ aa: Jase, gbuno kɔrɔ, gɩdonɩ gɩ teenanɛ dɩ ma cɔ afɩ cɔ nĩ.
42019006	Dɩ Jase gbũ kɔrɔ a teguu kpakpaalɛ na daʋ.
42019007	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ yɩnɩ gelela, wɩ-n hũhuune ayɩ: A jaal a cɔ sopugodaarɩ cɔ.
42019008	Sɩ Jase ɩɩr jɩɩl Kɔ̃tɩnɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa sʋʋraa: Hɩnɛ Kɔ̃tɩn, dakuru ɩ̃ thɩ̃sɔra ma-n har bɔdara. A mɩ kɔɔ tee tibil thɩ̃ɛ na fɩɩlɛ, ma bire na haa balanã.
42019009	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Taarɛ lʋʋn cʋɔrɔɔkɛ nĩ, gɩdonɩ Abɩrahamɩ bikuun olela do dakha.
42019010	Gɩdonɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ɩnɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ bonɩɩ ƴaal pa ɩ̃ taa wɩ.
42019011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ hanɩle dɩ wa-n pɛ Jeju nũu, a so warɛ sokpa bɩɛl wo, gɩdonɩ a wɔrɔnɛ Jerujalɛm dɩ wɩ kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar Thãgba na gbaar fãga dapa dapaara.
42019012	Dɩ a so warɛ: Nũfe kuun gɩ da-n jal dɩ kpɩɩra ƴɔɔ fh wɩ cʋgʋʋ a do fãgadaar, sɩ a bir a ɩ̃.
42019013	Dɩ a tire ɔɔ thɔ̃darasɔra tɩbɩla yʋɔr a ha wɩ war bɔrɔ bɩɛlbɩɛl sa so war: Na-n ƴabana phaphapha ma ɩnɛ.
42019014	Sɩ ɔɔ dɩdara n kɔɔ laarʋʋrɛ, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a jalnɩ pɩ, wɩ thʋɔn thɔ̃thɔna wɩ kpaanɛ a sɔ: Sa-n ƴaal olela a dɔ sar fãgadaara'.
42019015	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a 'lɛnɩ fãga pɩ, a kɛr bir ɩ̃. A wer thɔ̃daraakɛra a kɔɔ hanɩ war wɩ pɔ, a jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ wɛr bɩɛlbɩɛl 'lɛnɩ dɩɩ do khor.
42019016	Dɩ cacadaar pɔr a sor: Kɔ̃tɩn, afɩ bɔrɔ bɩɛl bire 'lɛr khor yʋɔι a dɛbɩrɔ wo.
42019017	Dɩ sʋʋraa: Gɩ bɔrɛ, thɔ̃daar bʋɔ ha fɩ. Gɩdonɩ fɩ dor sobɔ cʋʋdaar thɩ̃ gberakɛ, dɔ gobanɛr dɩɩ yʋɔrra.
42019018	Dɩ balanyɔdaar pɔ a so: Kɔ̃tɩn, afɩ bɔrɔ bɩɛlla bire 'lɛr khor yemɔɩ a dɛbɩrɔ wo.
42019019	Dɩ sʋʋraa: Na fɛrɛ dakha, fa dor gobanɛr dιι yemɔιra.
42019020	Dι bιɛl pɔ a so: Kɔ̃tιn, yɛ afι bɔrɔ bιɛlla kẽkẽ ballɔ mer kɔɔ to gι.
42019021	Gιdonι afιdara n kʋ mɛr maar gιdonι fι dor nĩkhidaar, dι fι gba gιrɛɛkɛ fa kɔɔ thιιnna', dι fι khana gιrɛɛkɛ fa kɔɔ diirnə'.
42019022	Dι sʋʋraa: Fɛr thɔ̃daar puukɛ, afɩ thɩmɩɩra ma gba a na kɩɩlna fɩ. Fɩ kɔɔ jɩnɩ dɩ nĩkhidaar ha mɩ, dɩ ɩ̃ gba gɩrɛɛkɛ ma kɔɔ thɩɩnna', dɩ ɩ̃ kha gɩrɛɛkɛ ma kɔɔ diirnə'.
42019023	Dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa kɔɔ 'laa ɩ̃ war kãkɛ ma 'lɛrɔnɩ khor a mɩ bir ɩ̃a?
42019024	Agɩpɩ a sor wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩle ayɩ: Nɩ taaraa bɔrɔ bɩɛlɩle, a hana ʋrɛ hananɩ bɔrɔ yʋɔr.
42019025	Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tιn, mee bɔrɔ yʋɔr a hana.
42019026	Mι so narɛ, tibil wo tibilikɛ hananι thɩ̃ɛ, wa bire na 'laa na dɛbιraa wo, sι tibilikɛ na hananι thɩ̃a', wa tiirəərerakɛ phubi gιrɛɛkɛ a hananι.
42019027	Sι ado ɩ̃ lãlaardarasɔɔkɛ na kɔɔ ƴaalɛ mιnι ɩ̃ dɔ war fãgadaara' wɛ, nι kpa wι ɛna a kʋʋrɛ ɩ̃ ƴɛra.
42019028	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju mιιnι thale pι, a kʋʋl wɛr ƴιɛ da-n jal Jerujalɛm.
42019029	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n wɔrɔnι Bɛtιfaje na Betanι khʋra, gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔkɛ hananι olιvι thιra, le a thɔ̃ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yenyɔ a so war ayι:
42019030	Nι jala dιιraakɛ nɩ pɛnɩ ƴɩɛ. A nɩ pɔ na dã, na yɩrɛ kũkə̃ ɓolʋʋkɛ tibil na jʋʋnnɩ pa' dɩ wa li. Nɩ thʋba a kpa ɛna.
42019031	A tibil bule ni: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n thʋbɩ ya? Nɩ sʋɔraa ayɛ: Kɔ̃tɩn n ƴaalɛ.
42019032	Dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ Jeju kɔɔ thɔnɩ jaal a yɩ thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ ha mɔna a kɔɔ so warnɩ.
42019033	Dɩ mɔ̃ wɩ-n thʋbɩnɩ kũkə̃ ɓolʋ, ɔɔ hɩ̃hɩ̃sɔ bule wer. Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n thʋbɩ kũkə̃ ɓolʋʋkɛ?
42019034	Dɩ wɩ birse: Kɔ̃tɩn n ƴaalɛ.
42019035	Dɩ wɩ pɔnanɛ kũkə̃ ɓolʋ Jejura, a gba awɩ kẽkẽ a dɛ̃ɛ kũkəənə, sa cʋʋ dɩ Jeju jʋʋn.
42019036	Mɔ̃ a-n jalnɩ, tɩbɩla kɔɔ belle awɩ kẽkẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ a pɛr hʋɛra.
42019037	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a thenɩ olɩvɩ thɩr gɔ̃gʋɔna a gbũ da-n dã, daʋ fʋrɛ kpãkpãada jɔjʋɔɔle fɛʋ, dɩ wɩ ma dɩ wa-n khɩɩ Thãgba na nɔ kheu nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ fɛʋraakɛ wɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ.
42019038	Dɩ wa-n so: “Bɔnanɛ n hana fãgadaarraakɛ n ɩnanɩ gɩrɛ na Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i. Ha ɩɩ n hana Thãgbaa dʋɔ na i dʋbɩrɛ thãgbara ƴũ pər.”
42019039	Ɩkhaa jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thɩɩn kɔɔ sor Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, phaanɛ afɩ kpãkpãadara.
42019040	Dɩ birse wi: Mɩ so narɛ a wɩrɛ pɩr nʋɔrakɛ, bokanasɔ na-n hulene.
42019041	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n kɔɔ wɔrɔnɩ a 'laa na yɩ dɩɩle, a-n khɩɩrɛ sa so:
42019042	Fɛrɛ Jerujalɛm dakha, adora fɩ jɩrɛ gɩrɛ nĩ wireraakɛ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ na hana fɩnɩna ha ɩɩ, sɩ hɩnɛ nɛnɛ̃, gɩ ker farɛ gɩrɛ waa.
42019043	Wire na phã farɛ kɛ afɩ lãlaardara na kpenɩ koru a na dii far, sɩ na kpala far a na sɔbɩ fɩ paar fɛʋ kpɩkpɩkpɩ.
42019044	Dɩ wa cɛcɛbɛ fɛr koo na afɩ bɩsãsɔɔkɛ hanɩ afɩ kal ƴɔɔ, dɩ wa sɩ far boka bɩɛl a dɛ̃ɛ bɩɛlla ga, gɩdonɩ fa kɔɔ jɩ bɔɔkɛ Thãgba kher fɩna'.
42019045	Dɩ Jeju lõ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, a ma a weele wɩrɛ n dolonenɩ thɩ̃ɛ,
42019046	sa so war: Gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Mɛr Thãgbaa cɔ na dor ɩ̃ fʋɔr pa”, sι dι ne wer cʋʋ dɩɩ do yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaraa wɔ̃ pa.
42019047	Dɩ Jeju n kɔɔ hale da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla wire fɛʋ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna. Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara na tɩbɩlaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ n kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ kʋʋ.
42019048	Sɩ wa jɩ mɔ̃ wa cʋʋnɩ sɩ na fʋʋa', gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ nũu bɔɔbɔɔbɔɔ.
42020001	Dɩ wi bɩɛl mɔ̃kɛ Jeju n kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, da-n mɩɩna wɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tιna na jɔfʋ dιιrdara na kɔ̃tιna pɔr
42020002	a bulee: Sɔ sar ka hʋ caakɛra fι hananι dι fa-n cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛɛkɛra thenι, dι amɛ dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ hana fιnι hʋɛɛkɛra? Dι birse wi:
42020003	Ma bule ner mer dakha thɩ̃ bιɛl.
42020004	Nι sɔ mar: Jãa yɔ kpɛɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ gι the yaa, tιbιlaa pa gι the?
42020005	Dι wι mar dι wa-n bana kha awι hasɔ ayι: Ado sι tu ayι: Thãgbaa dʋɔ gι the, a na bule ser dι anye dɔ kιrʋ dι sa kɔɔ pɛ ɔɔ thιmιι haara'.
42020006	Dι ado sι tu wo ayι: Tιbιlaa pa gι the, tιbιla fɛʋ na dʋʋr sɛr na bokana, gιdonι wι jιɛ jι dι Thãgbaa bobon Jã kɔɔ do.
42020007	Dι wι birse: Sa jι ka gι thena'.
42020008	Dι Jeju so war: Dι a thale gι, mɛrɛ dakha ma so nar ka mι yιnι hʋɛ dι ma-n cʋʋna ga thɩ̃sɔɔka'.
42020009	Agιpι Jeju gbaar thιmιιr a mιι tιbιla na sokpaa ayι: Kũu bιɛl gι, a kɔɔ cʋʋ nãkʋɔr a gba nãkʋɔr hιιndara a pɛr wa-n hιnɛ ɓo, sa jal kpaar paar da-n pʋɔr.
42020010	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ bi khʋ̃ bɔɔ danι, a thʋɔn ɔɔ thɔ̃daar bιɛl a jala nãkʋɔr hιιndarara wι hanaa dιkhaa nãkʋɔr thιr bi a pɔna. Sι nãkʋɔr hιιndara bιιrʋʋrɛ sa weguu dι kɔna nyɛ̃ biire.
42020011	Dι bir thɔ̃ thɔ̃daar kpιι wo, dι wι bιιrʋʋ a pιɛraa yicuru dι kɔna nyɛ̃ biire.
42020012	Dι bir thɔ̃ balãtherdaar wo, dι wι pιɛraa kaar sa weguu.
42020013	Dι nãkʋɔr kɔ̃tιn so: Anye ma cʋʋ dιphã ya fɛ? Ɩ̃ bikuunikɛ mι-n nanι ma thɔ̃. Agakpaana ɔr wa cʋ.
42020014	Sι ɔbɔɔkɛ nãkʋɔr hιιndara yιιnι, wι mιιrɛ kha awι ha ayι: Ʋrɛ dʋɔn thɩ̃ hιn, nι dɔ sι kʋʋ sι thɩ̃ɛ n do asιda.
42020015	Dι wι gbaa a dʋna nãkʋɔr khuirə sa kʋʋ. Anye nãkʋɔr kɔ̃tιn na cʋʋ wι dιphã?
42020016	A na pɔr na kʋʋr nãkʋɔr hιιndaraale sa a gba nãkʋɔr a ha tιι kpιιsɔ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ wι nιɛnι gele wι sor: Ga-n ha thala koe.
42020017	Sι Jeju na-n hιιn wι sa so war: Dι anye gιrɛɛkɛ kherenenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ƴaal gι so: “Bokaarιkɛ cɔ mɛ kɔɔ bonι debire a do go tι bokaar”?
42020018	Dι tibil wo tibilikɛ na jenι bokaarraakɛ a na khaarɛ, sι tibil wo tibilikɛ bokaarιkɛ na jironi, ga cʋ̃banʋʋnɛ pɛrɛ pɛrɛ.
42020019	Dι bonι jidaar kɔ̃tιna na jɔfʋ dιιrdara n kɔɔ ƴaalɛ hʋɛ wɩ fʋ Jeju dabɔɔlera, sιι do maar n fʋ wɛr tιbιlala. Gιdonι wι kɔɔ jιrɛ dι wɛrra Jeju so sokpaale.
42020020	Dɩ wɩ mar dɩ wa-n jʋʋr Jeju, a thʋɔnaa gɩgɩla dɩ wɩ pɛr fɩɩlɛ dɩɩ ho tɩɩ sara wɩ do, sɩ wɩ nʋɔ wι fʋ thɩmιιrra, wι liirnaa wι to fãga paar gobanɛr nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
42020021	Dι wι buleele: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ jɩrɛ fɩ-n mɩɩrɛ dɩ fa-n dɩɩrna tɩbɩla gɩrɛ dɔnɩ sobɔr, dɩ fa-n hɩɩn dakha tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa' sɩ dɩ fa-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla Thãgbaa hʋ na sobɔr.
42020022	Gɩ teere kha dɩ sa lɩmɩ Sejaar lãpho yaa, ga tee kha ga?
42020023	Sɩ Jeju jɩrɛ awɩ fɩɩl, a birse wi: Nɩ nɛna mɩ war bire ɩ̃ hɩɩn.
42020024	Amɛ ha ʋrɛ fotoraakɛ? Dɩ amɛɛ khere ha gɩrɛ? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Sejaar gɩ.
42020025	Dɩ Jeju so war: Dɩ gɛr gɩ nɩ 'laanɛ Sejaarra gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Sejaarɩda, a 'laanɛ Thãgbara gɩrɛ dɔhɩ Thãgbaada.
42020026	Dι wa kɔɔ puno a na fʋʋrakɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ bɩɛlla tɩbɩlaa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩna', sɩ nʋɔ ka kɔɔ kpaa wɛr mɔ̃ a birse wini dɩ wɩ pɩr dɩphã pɔbɩ.
42020027	Dɩ ɩkhaa Sadʋsɛ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala' pʋɔraarɛ, a bulee thakɛ aa:
42020028	Dɩɩrdaar, hɩnɛ gɩrɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ khere sarnɩ: “Ado tibil hana õkuun dɩ khi sa faa khɛr sɩ bɩsaan na hala', ɔɔ õkuun n gba hɛ a kɔna bɩsana wɩ do ɔɔ õkuuni məl.”
42020029	Dɩ õkona makonyɔ wɛ a kɔɔ hale, dɩ cacadaar kɔɔ her khɛr aa hana bɩsana ga, sa khi.
42020030	Dɩ balanyɔdaar na balãtherdaar gbaar khikhɛrʋʋlera.
42020031	Mɛna gɩ hana wɛr makonyɔɔle fɛʋ kɔɔ khireni, sɩ wa hana bɩsaana'.
42020032	Agɩpɩ khɛrɩlera dakha khire.
42020033	Dɩ ado khe na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera, ʋmɔ̃ wɛrra na hɩna khɛrɩle? Gɩdonɩ wɛr makonyɔra fɛʋʋ khɛr a kɔɔ do.
42020034	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ bɩsãsɔ n her khɛra, dɩ khɛra n her kona.
42020035	Sɩ wɩrɛ wa yɩnɩ, wɛr teana a na 'lɛ awɩda bɔɔraalera na ɩnanɩ a na ɩɩrna dakha na the khirera, wɛr wa he khɛra ga, dɩ khɛra na he kona ga.
42020036	Dɩ wa puno a na khi dakha bã, gɩdonι wa hʋrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ a na do Thãgbaa bιsãsɔ, gιdonι wι ɩɩrɛ a the khirera.
42020037	Dɩ ado khee ɩɩr gɩ, gɛr dɔ gιrɛ Mʋιjι kɔɔ cʋʋnι dι sι jι thɩr bu thιmιιrra, ɔbɔɔkɛ a wenι Kɔ̃tιn, “Abιrahamι Thãgba, na Ɩjakιι Thãgba, na Jakɔbιι Thãgba”.
42020038	Sι Thãgba na do khee Thãgba ga, sι wιrɛ hananι yiree Thãgba a do, gιdonɩ ado ɔrra gɩ, tιbιla fɛʋ hananɛ yire.
42020039	Dι ιkhaa jɔfʋ dιιrdara birsee: Dιιrdaar, sobɔr fι mιι.
42020040	Dι wa 'la na bulee thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ bã.
42020041	Dι Jeju bule wi: Mɔ̃ gι fʋ sι tιbιla na-n so aa: Davιdιι Bikuun Kirisiti do?
42020042	Davιdιι thɛthɛ kɔɔ sor Khιkhιι nι sɛbɛra ayι: “Thãgba sor ɩ̃ Kɔ̃tιna ayι: Tɔɔ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra,
42020043	phaphapha ɩ̃ cʋʋ afι lãlaardara wι do afι nɛ jəəda.”
42020044	Dι a Davιdι n wιιrɛ Kɔ̃tιn thale, mɔ̃ a na fʋ sι na do ɔɔ bikuun?
42020045	Mɔna tιbιla fɛʋ n kɔɔ pιɛnι nũu, a sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayι:
42020046	Na-n jιɛ dʋ bʋrɛ jɔfʋ dιιrdarasɔraakɛ n ƴaalɛnι ιnι-n tɔ kẽkẽ gbana a na kpaarna ƴatɔɔ, kɛ n naannι tιbιlasɔ na-n fʋɔrɛnι kɔ̃tɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋ, kɛ n phireni ƴɛ kʋʋl too paar Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ, na ƴɛ kʋʋl too paar dιko kho paar,
42020047	kɛ n phʋʋnɛnɩ khikhɛra, sɩɩ do fɩɩlɛ wɩ-n bɩɛlna Thãgba dɩ wa-n pʋɔrna wa-n yɛ nɩ. Wele so kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na heen wer na khɩɩr na ka.
42021001	Dɩ Jeju gba da-n hɩɩn a yɩ lɛ̃lɛɛkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ war Thãgba mũsũ pɛ paar.
42021002	Dɩ le a yɩ dakha khikhɛr bɔdaar dɩ pɔna tama be yenyɔ a pɛr.
42021003	Dɩ so: Sobɔr mɩ so nar, khikhɛr bɔdaarɩkɛ pɛrɛ war Thãgba mũsũ pɛ paar dɩɩ jɔ wɛr fɛʋ.
42021004	Gɩdonɩ war harra wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ pɛr war Thãgba mũsũ pɛ paar, sɩ ɔr, ɔɔ bɔdaar warɩkɛ na haanɛɛnɩ a gba koo a pɛr.
42021005	Mɔ̃kɛ ɩkhasɔ n kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ boka ɓɔna na khaardaasɔɔkɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dɩɩ ɓɔ̃ kaada, Jeju so warɛ ayɩ:
42021006	Bɔɔ na daan dɩ gɩrɛɛkɛra nɩ yɩnɩ, boka bɩɛl na bir na sɩ a na dɛ̃ɛ ʋ̃ bokara ƴũ bã, sɩ fɛʋ na derre.
42021007	Dι wι bulee: Dιιrdaar, ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ gelela na dã? Dι anye dɔ jιιnιkɛ na nɛnanι bɔɔkɛ gelesɔra na-n danι?
42021008	Dι Jeju birse wi: Na-n jιɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, na-n do tibil n fιιl na', gιdonι tιbιla bərəəm na gbaar ɩ̃ i na ιna wa-n sona wι yι, ιnɛr dʋɔn mɛrɛ; dι wo, bɔɔ n daan. Na-n ha na kpa wara' koe.
42021009	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ na nιɛnι kʋʋr hale na lãʋsɔ, na-n do maar n fʋ na', gιdonι dɔ gele n kɔɔ dã ɓo, sι ga do gɛr na dʋɔn thι pι paar dapaara pa'.
42021010	Le a so war: Ʋ ca na ιιrɛ a na-n khena ʋ̃ ca, dι ʋ̃ fãgadaarι dι bιɛl na ιιrɛ a na-n kena ʋ̃ fãgadaarι dι kpιι.
42021011	Dι thι jẽ kɔ̃tιna, na kho mananɛsɔ, na kɔmɛ kɔ̃tιnasɔ na hale paar dιιdιιsɔ. Hərə thɩ̃ɛ na nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kɔ̃tιnasɔɔkɛ thɛnι ƴũ na hale dakha.
42021012	Sι gιrɛ na kʋlɛnι gele ƴιɛ, tιbιla na fʋlɛ nɛr wa-n kpoo nar. Wa fʋlɛ nɛr na jalna Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ na khaι cɔnanɔ. Wa kpa nɛr na jalna fãgadarara na gobanɛrsɔɔ ƴɛra, gι do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ.
42021013	Gɛr na yιrɔ hʋɛ a na mιι wι anι sobɔ so jι thιmιι.
42021014	Gɛr gι na-n jɛna gι dι na-n ha na kɔɔ dɛ anye na so yaa ga.
42021015	Gιdonι mɛr na sɔ nar gιrɛɛkɛ na mιιnι, ɩ̃ hana nι kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ anι lãlaardarasɔ fɛʋ na punoni a na mara', agιbo a na bana ga.
42021016	Anι thιrakɛ, na anι nι, na anι õkuunsɔ, na anι too, na anι kuunsɔ, wa liirna nɛr, dι wa cʋʋrɛ ιkhaa tibilsɔ anι thɩ̃thιιn dι wa khiir.
42021017	Tιbιla fɛʋ na-n laar nɛr gι do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ.
42021018	Sι anι yʋsũ bιɛllakɛ na 'la na buə'.
42021019	A nɩ yιr, na 'lɛr taarɛ.
42021020	Ɔbɔɔkɛ na yιnι sɔrasɛsɔ dι wa kpala Jerujalɛm dιιra, nι jɛ gι do ɔɔ bũburõ bɔ n daan.
42021021	Le wιrɛ hanι Jude n fuo ca jala gɔ̃gʋɔna, wιrɛ hanι Jerujalɛm dι bιnɔ n ιrɛ na thɛ, wιrɛ hanι kõgosora na lõ dι bιnɔ bã.
42021022	Gιdonι ga wisɔɔle na do wiresɔɔkɛ Thãgba na tiirni helu, gι cʋʋ gιrɛ kherenenι fɛʋ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra gι dã.
42021023	Ga wisɔɔle, ga puurore khɛ pɛmɛdarara na wιrɛ n mamanι bibɔrɔsɔ. Gιdonι nι kɔ̃tɩ̃ι na hale dιιraale na Thãgbaa nĩkhiikɛ na-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛnanι ga tibil caakɛ.
42021024	Bajιna na kʋʋrɛ wɩ, wa fʋlɛ wɛr na jalna wɩ do dea ca kpalaa dɩra fɛʋ, dɩ Jerujalɛm na dor ca kpalaa nɛ saar pa phaphapha ca kpalaa bɔ n dã.
42021025	Jιιnsɔ na hale wirera na porra na ƴepələ̃besɔra; sι kɛkɛ thιιra bɔ gaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ι na hale tibil caarra fɛʋ, kɛ na jɛnι mɔ̃ wa donι lanyʋɔnnaakɛ n uboni dι a-n bɛɛna ga.
42021026	Tιbιla na khiire maarra mɔ̃ wι-n kpιɛrnanι gɩrɛɛkɛ na dananɩ thɩɩra, gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ fãgaakɛ hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ ga gbugbuyore.
42021027	Le wa yɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun ma-n ɩna ndɔlɔ̃paar, na fãga, na carbarɛ jɔɔ.
42021028	Ɔbɔɔkɛ gelela na tɔ̃tʋɔnnɩ ga-n dã, nɩ jɩɛ jɩɩl sa gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ na hɩnɛ, gɩdonɩ anɩ birse bɔ n daan.
42021029	Dɩ Jeju so war sokpa bɩɛl ayɩ: Nɩ hɩnɛ thɩr khonanɛ na thɩrasɔɔkɛ fɛʋ.
42021030	Ɔbɔɔkɛ awɩ fasɔ n thɔɔnɩ, nɩ jɩrɛ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛrakɛ dɩ ubulo wɩllɛ pɩ.
42021031	Dɩ mɛ̃ gɩ nɛrɛ dakha, a nɩ yɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ dɩ a dã, nɩ jɛ dɩ Thãgbaa fãga gba bɔ daan.
42021032	Sobɔr mɩ so nar, nĩdaraakɛ na khiir koo sɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ fɛʋ na dã ga.
42021033	Thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩ na phor na ka, sɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔ na pho na ka kpɩɩraka'.
42021034	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, dɩ kɛbɩrɛ, na ta laarɛ, na dɛrɩkɛ dɔnɩ thɩɩkɛɛda na-n cʋʋ nɩ dɩ na jʋʋr bã, dι ga wiile na danι gι ho mɔ̃kɛ pheru n cιna'.
42021035	Gιdonι mɛ̃ wireele na phã tιbιlala fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ thɩɩra.
42021036	Gɛr gɩ na-n jʋrɛ a na bɩɛlna Thãgba bɔɔ fɛʋ, a 'lɛ fãga a fuona gɩrɛraakɛra fɛʋ na dananɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ na jɩɩl mɛr tibili Bikuuni ƴɛra.
42021037	Hɩwɛra Jeju n kɔɔ hale Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla, sɩ a dɩɩ tɩ̃, dɩ jal dɩ cɔ olɩvɩ thɩr gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ.
42021038	Sɩ jijiirə tɩbɩla fɛʋ n pʋɔraarɛ le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, dɩ wa-n pɩɛ nũu.
42022001	Fɛtɩɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pakɩ, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraada n wɔrɔnɛ.
42022002	Le bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara n kɔɔ ƴaal hʋɛ mɔ̃ wa cʋʋnɩ sɩ wɩ kʋ Jeju, gɩdonɩ maar n fʋɔn wɩ tɩbɩlala.
42022003	Dɩ Satã lõ Judasɩraakɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ, ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ kpãkpãadaar bɩɛl yʋɔr yenyɔra.
42022004	Dɩ a jaal a gʋʋrna bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ gardɛɛ kʋmãdasɔ mɔ̃ a na cʋʋnɩ sɩ na liirna Jeju na ha wɩ.
42022005	Dɩɩ da war na sobɔr dɩ wɩ yɩ, ɩna haarɛ war.
42022006	Dɩ tu a jɩɩ ma da-n ƴaal hʋɛ waa a liirna wɩ Jeju, sɩ tibil jɔ na ja'.
42022007	Dɩ buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraa fɛtɩ wi dã, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ wireekɛ wɩ-n jinəni Pakɩ bana bire bonɩɛ.
42022008	Dɩ Jeju thɔ̃ Pɩɛr na Jã a so war ayɩ: Nɩ jala a gbɛbɩrɛ sar Pakɩ dɩkor dɩ sa kho.
42022009	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Kana fɩ-n ƴaal dɩ sa gbɛbɩ?
42022010	Dɩ birse wi: Nɩ hɩnɛ, ɔbɔɔkɛ na lonɩ dɩɩra, kuunikɛ heenenɩ nyʋɔn na daa na caana nɛr. Na-n kpaaraa cʋɔrraakɛ a na lonɩ;
42022011	dɩ nɩ sɔ cɔdaar kuunna: Dɩɩrdaar n bule fer aa, kana duu na ha dɩ ɩna khoro Pakɩ dɩkor na ɩnɩ kpãkpãadara ya?
42022012	Dɩ a na nɩ narɛ lɩ̃gã kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ wɩ thɩɩnɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ. Le na gbɛbɩrɩ Pakɩ dɩkor.
42022013	Dɩ wɩ jaal a yɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ ha mɔna Jeju kɔɔ so warnɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ gbɛbɩ Pakɩ dɩkor.
42022014	Ɔbɔɔkɛ bɔɔ danɩ, Jeju toore dɩko kho paar na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔnaakɛ wɩ hananɩ kha.
42022015	Dɩ a so warɛ ayɩ: Mɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ na ɩ̃ ha fɛʋ dɩ ma kho Pakɩ dɩkorɩkɛ na nɛrɛ ɓo sɩ bɔ gaarɛ n dã mɩ.
42022016	Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ: Ma bir na kho Pakɩ dɩkorɩkɛ kpɩɩ bã, phaphapha gɩrɛ gelela ƴaalnɩ gɩ so n yɩr casɩ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
42022017	Dɩ a gbaar thɩ̃ yɔnanɛ a bɩɛl Thãgba pɛr sa so: Nɩ gba thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ a tɩnɛnɛ anɩ ha.
