42022018	Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ: Ma bir na yɔ dɩvɛ̃ bã, phaphapha Thãgba n gba fãga.
42022019	Agɩpɩ dɩ gba buru. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a kuure a ha wɩ sa so: Gɩrɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ tomɩɩkɛ [mɩ 'laanɩ ha nɩ, na-n cʋɛ thakɛ a na jɛna mɩ.
42022020	Dɩ mɛ̃ a cʋʋ na thɩ̃ yɔnanɛ dakha. Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ khonɩ dɩkor pɩ, a ha wɛr sa so: Thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ dʋɔn nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ phaakɛ thɛnɩ ɩ̃ tɔmɩnaakɛ na deerenɩ nɛrɛɛ sora.]
42022021	Sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, ʋrɛɛkɛ na lirena mɩnɩ hakɛ dɩko kho paar na mɛrɛ.
42022022	Mɛr tibili Bikuun n jaal mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba pɛrnɩ gɩ hana. Sɩ ga puure tibilləəkɛ na lirena mɩnɩ.
42022023	Dɩ wɩ ma dɩ wa-n bule kha bɩɛlbɩɛl awɩ ha ayɩ, amɛ ɩnɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn na cʋɛ ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ?
42022024	Thɩ̃ banaa kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ dakha awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ wa-n bana kha awɩ ha aa: Amɛ asɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn teana gɩrɛra a dɔ kɔ̃tɩn ya fɛ?
42022025	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ca kpalaa fãgadara n ʋʋnɛ tɩbɩlala kpɛ, dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ hananɩ fãga wɛrra n cʋʋrɛ dɩ wa-n we wɩ bɔ cʋʋdara.
42022026	Sɩ ga teena gɩ hana mɛ̃ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩnaa koe; sɩ tibilikɛ kanɩ do kɔ̃tɩn anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɔ ɔr n ka a do dabuu, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ yʋʋ, dɔ ɔr n ka a do thɔ̃daar.
42022027	Gɩdonɩ ʋmɔ̃ n dɔ kɔ̃tɩn, ʋrɛɛkɛ n tɔɔnɩ dɩko kho paar gɩ yaa, agɩbo ʋrɛɛkɛ n tɩnɛnɛnɩ gɩ? Ga do ʋrɛɛkɛ n tɔɔnɩ dɩko kho paar gaa? Sɩ mɛrɛ, mɩ ka har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a ho thɔ̃daar.
42022028	Nɛrɛ, nɛr dʋɔn wɩrɛɛkɛ jɩlɛ marnɩ kɩbɩ ɩ̃ bɔ gaarra.
42022029	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ thɩɩn Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩ anɩ thɩɩn, mɔ̃kɛ ɩ̃ Thɩ kɔɔ thɩɩn gɩnɩ ɩ̃ thɩɩn;
42022030	dɩ mɛ̃ na kho na-n yɔna ɩ̃ dɩko kho para ɩ̃ fãgadaarɩ dɩra, nɩ too dakha fãga too paarsɔ na-n kɩɩlna Ɩjɩrayɛl ca yʋɔr yenyɔ.
42022031	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn so aa: Sɩmɔ̃, Sɩmɔ̃, hɩnɛ Satã n kɔɔ luure ka ɩnɩ-n jɛ nɩ jʋ khaa.
42022032	Sɩ mɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ Thãgba a pɛ far dɩ afɩ ha pɛ na-n buə', sɩ fɛrɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ fa kɛrnɩ na bir Thãgbara, cʋɛ afɩ omisɔ wɩ tɩ.
42022033	Dɩ Pɩɛr sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tιn, mι gbɛbιrɛ pι dι sa lõ kha khaιra, dι ma khi dakha na fɛrɛ.
42022034	Sι Jeju sʋʋraa: Pɩɛr, mɩ so farɛ yɔl kʋʋ na khɩɩ nĩkɛ pa', sɩ balãther fa bana nayɩ fa jɩ ma'.
42022035	Dɩ Jeju bule wer wo ayɩwɔɔ: Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ thɔ̃ nɩnɩ sɩ na kɔɔ hana pɔtɩma, dɩ lokaar gɩ dɩ nɛfaa ga, thɩ̃ɛ kɔɔ ɓɔr nɛr ya? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Thɩ̃ bιɛllakɛ na kɔɔ ɓɔr sa'.
42022036	Dι so war: Sι nɛnɛ̃kɛ ga ha mã'. Tibilikɛ hananɩ pɔtɩma, dɔ a gba a fʋrɔ, mɛna gɩ na tibilikɛ hananɩ lokaar. Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ bajɩna ga, dɔ a dolõ ɔɔ kẽkẽ a thena bajɩna.
42022037	Gɩdonɩ mɩ so narɛ, gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ kherenenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra teenanɛ gɩ dã mɩ, gɩ sor: “Wɩ kɔɔ theruure a ɓã puu cʋʋdarara.” Dɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ ba mɩnɩɩ bɔɔ n daan.
42022038	Dɩ wɩ so: Kɔ̃tɩn hɩnɛ, bajɩna yenyɔ hakɛ; dɩ birse wi: Gɩ daan.
42022039	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ thenɩ, a jaal olɩvɩ thɩr gɔ̃gʋɔna mɔ̃kɛ a mɩlna gɩnɩ. Ɔɔ kpãkpãadara kpaaraarɛ.
42022040	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ danɩ paarɩle, a so warɛ ayɩ: Nɩ bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba dɩ mɛ̃ na lõ fifiləlela ga.
42022041	Agɩpɩ Jeju tɔ jal ƴɔɔ gbe dɩɩ mãkha na mɔ̃kɛ tibil n dʋnanɩ bokaar dɩɩ dã, a gburõku da-n bɩɛl Thãgba da-n sona:
42022042	Thɩrɛ, ado fɩ-n ƴaalɛ hʋnɔnɛ mar thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ, sɩ ga do mɔ̃ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ ga, sɩ mɔ̃ fɛrɛ n pɛrnɩ haar gɩ hana.
42022043	[Dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl ther Thãgbaa dʋɔ a pɔ a haa fãga.
42022044	Sɩ mɔ̃ Jeju hanɩ da-n 'wãga, a yɩrrɛ a jɩɩ bɩɛl Thãgba dɩ ga-n pɛr; dɩ ɔɔ hʋ̃ʋsɛɛkɛ a hʋ̃ʋsɛnɩ thʋ̃ debi a ho tɔmɩn dɩ ga-n 'lũ thɩɩra.]
42022045	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba pɩ, a ɩɩrɛ a bir pɔ kpãkpãadaraa pa, a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa-n daar gɩdonɩ wɩ gbobire.
42022046	Dɩ bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n daar? Nɩ ɩrɛ a na bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba dɩ mɛ̃ na lõ fifiləlela ga.
42022047	Mɔ̃ Jeju hanɩ mɩɩrɔ, hɩnɛ tibil jɔ kɔɔ daan. Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Judasɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ bɩɛl kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔra kʋlɛ wɩ ƴɩɛ, a tɔ pɔ Jejura a palʋʋ.
42022048	Dɩ Jeju bulee: Judasɩ, pallɛla fɩ liirna mɛr tibili Bikuun bɛɛ?
42022049	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ hanɩ kha na Jeju kɔɔ yɩnɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ n dananɩ, wɩ buleele: Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩ cɛna bajɩna ya?
42022050	Dɩ bɩɛl wɛrra cɩrɛ gbõdaarɩ thɔ̃daar nyɔ̃bɔ nũu a kʋr.
42022051	Sɩ Jeju bir so: Na-n cʋʋ thakɛ bã, sa thar kuuni nunəəle dɩɩ ba.
42022052	Agɩpɩ Jeju so bonɩ jida kɔ̃tɩnasɔra, na Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ gardɛɛ kʋmãdasɔra, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔraakɛ kɔɔ pʋɔnnɩ wɩ fʋʋ ayɩ: Nɩ ɩnanɛ bajɩna na gbolasɔ nɩ fʋ mɩ, mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n fʋnɩ yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaar koe.
42022053	Mɩ-n kɔɔ har kha na nɛrɛ wire fɛʋ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, sɩ na kɔɔ tha mar nyɔ̃a'. Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ dʋɔn anɩ bɔ dã pa, na dabirəə fãga bɔ.
42022054	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ fʋnɩ Jeju pɩ, wɩ kpaarɛ jalna gbõdaarɩ cɔ, sɩ Pɩɛr n kpar Jejura nɔ bɩɛl nɔ bɩɛl.
42022055	Dɩ tɩbɩla kɔɔ gbɔɔrɛ dɔɔ gbaya thɩ̃thɩɩn a tooro, dɩ Pɩɛr kɔɔ toore kha na wɛr.
42022056	Dɩ thɔ̃daar khɛ bɩɛl yɩɩ dɩ too a wɔrɔ̃ dɔɔ, dɩ hɩɩnʋʋ kirkirkir sa so aa: Kuunikɛ dakha kɔɔ har kha na ɔr.
42022057	Sɩ a bananɛ da-n sona ayɩ: Khɛr, ma jɩa'.
42022058	Bɔɔ gbe tibil kpɩɩ yɩɩ a so: Fɛrɛ dakha, wa tibil ca bɩɛl fɩ do. Dɩ Pɩɛr birsee: Kuun, ma do wa tibil ca ga.
42022059	A lɩɛr bɩɛl ka wo, tibil kpɩɩ borrakɛ da-n ɩɩraa ayɩ: Sobɔr gɩ gel, kuunikɛ kɔɔ har kha na Jeju gɩdonɩ Galiledaar a do.
42022060	Sɩ Pɩɛr sʋʋraa: Kuun, ma jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ fɩ-n ƴaalnɩ fɩ soa'. Dɩ mɔna a hanɩ mɩɩrɔ 'lo, dapaara yɔl kʋʋ khɩɩrɛ.
42022061	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn kɩɩl a hɩɩnʋʋ. Dɩ Pɩɛr jɩna thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ sʋʋraanɩ ayɩ: Yɔl kʋʋ na 'lɛ na khɩɩ nĩkɛ pa', sɩ fa bananɛ balãther nayɩ fa jɩ ma'.
42022062	Dɩ Pɩɛr the khuirə da-n bɩ sɔsɔsɔ.
42022063	Tɩbɩlaakɛ n bɛranɩ Jeju wɩ-n maanʋʋnɛ dɩ wa-n bɩɩrnaa,
42022064	a thii ƴɩɛ, sɩ wa-n bulee: Jɛ ntɛɛkɛ n bɛ fɩnɩ.
42022065	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ i kʋɛ thɩmɩa jɔɔjɔɔ a pɩɛraa.
42022066	A dɩɩ wɩl, tibil kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ kɔɔ kpar kha jɛ, sɩ dɩ wɩ kpa Jeju a pɔna awɩ so gʋʋrdarasɔɔ ƴɛra.
42022067	Dɩ wa-n bulee: Ado fɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti, sɔ sar. Dɩ Jeju birse wi: A mɩ so narrakɛ na pɛ gɩ haara'.
42022068	Dɩ a mɩ bule ni thɩ̃ɛ na tuə'.
42022069	Sɩ a fʋna nɛnɛ̃kɛ dɩphã, mɛr tibili Bikuun na toore Thãgbaa fãga nyɔ̃bɔra.
42022070	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ bulee: A thɩɛna ga, Thãgbaa Bikuun ha fɩ bɛɛ? Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sobɔr nɩ so, gɛr mɩ do ger.
42022071	Dɩ wɩ so: Dɩ anye hale dɩ sa bir na 'lo dɩkha 'lo, gɩdonɩ asɩ thɛthɛ nɩɛrɛ dɩ mɩɩna ɔɔ nɔ.
42023001	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ ɩɩr a kpa Jeju a jalna Pɩlatɩɩ ƴɛra,
42023002	a ma dɩ wa-n pɩɛraa sor ayɩ: Kuunikɛ sɩ fʋnɩ asɩ too a-n tɔ da-n pɛr laʋna, dɩ pɩɛrna tɩbɩla dakha wo wa-n lɩmɩ Sejaarɩ lãphoa', dɩ a kɔɔ sor dakha wo ayɩ, ιnɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti fãgadaar.
42023003	Dι Pιlatι bulee thakɛ: Fɛr dʋɔn Juifi fãgadaarι? Dι Jeju birsee: Mɔna fɩ sonɩ gɩ.
42023004	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ so bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnana, na tibil jɔraale ayɩ: Ma yɩ dɩ paar fɩɩʋrakɛ kuunnaaka'.
42023005	Sɩ wɩ bor dɩ wa-n so aa: A-n tɔr tɩbɩla da-n pɛr laʋna, da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla Jude dɩɩra fɛʋ, a fʋna Galile ka a kɔɔ fʋnɩ a dana kɩɛr.
42023006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pɩlatɩ nɩɛnɩ gele, a bulele ado kuunikɛ Galiledaar a do.
42023007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pɩlatɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩ Ɛrɔɔdιι marra Jeju the, a thɔnaanɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩraakɛ kɔɔ hanɩ Jerujalɛm dawiilera dakha.
42023008	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ Jeju daʋ fʋʋrɛ dɩɩ ka, gɩdonɩ gɩ maanɛ ka a kɔɔ ƴaalnɩ a yɩɩ, gɩrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ ɔɔda. Dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ pɛrɛ haar, ɩnɩ-n yɩɛ a cʋʋna dιkhaa nɔ kpaa thɩ̃.
42023009	Dι Ɛrɔɔdɩ buleele thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ, sɩ Jeju na kɔɔ birsee thɩ̃ bɩɛllaka'.
42023010	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ kɔɔ hale dɩ wa-n pɩɛraa sor na fãga.
42023011	Sɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ na ɔɔ sɔrasɩsɔ n kpɔ̃kpɔrɔɔnɛ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ maanʋʋnɩ sa tʋʋ kẽkẽ ɓʋ̃ɔ, Ɛrɔɔdɩ bire thɔnaa Pɩlatɩɩ pa wo.
42023012	Ga wiilera Ɛrɔɔdɩ na Pɩlatɩɩkɛ kɔɔ dɔnɩ kha lãlaardara mamara kũu kha dɩphã.
42023013	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ we bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na tɩbɩla a so war:
42023014	Nι kɔɔ ɩna marɛ kuunikɛ ayɩ, tɩbɩla a-n tɔ da-n pɛr laʋna; sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, mɩ kɔɔ buleele anɩ ƴɛra, dɩ ma yɩ puure kuunnaakɛra nɩ-n sonɩ gɩra'.
42023015	Ɛrɔɔdɩ dakha na kɔɔ yɩɩraa dɩ paara', gɩdonɩ a bire thɔnaa asɩ ƴɛra wo. Dɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, kuunikɛ na cʋʋ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ dɩɩ teena wɩ kʋʋa'.
42023016	A mɛ̃ gɩ khasa ma ciilnəə sɩ na fagʋʋ.
42023017	[Sɩ fɛtɩ bɔɔ fɛʋ Pɩlatɩ teenanɛ a faa khaɩdaarɩkɛ tɩbɩla n ƴaalnɩ a ha wɩ.]
42023018	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ hulẽ nɔ bɩɛl ayɩ: Cʋɛ kuunikɛ a khi, sɩ fι faa Barabasι fι ha sι.
42023019	Sι wι kɔɔ khaanɛ Barabasιιkɛ khaιra, gιdonι ɔr gιιkɛ ιrɛnanι lãʋ dι bιnɔ dι a kɔɔ kʋrɛ dakha tibil.
42023020	Dι mɔ̃kɛ Pιlatι kɔɔ pɛrnι haar ιnι-n faa Jeju, a bire bule tibil jɔɔle wo.
42023021	Sι wι hulene kheu aa: Gbaanɛɛ kpa kʋkʋ thιrʋra, gbaanɛɛ kpa kʋkʋ thιrʋra.
42023022	Dι Pɩlatɩ bir bule wi wo balãtherdaa: Anyee puu ca a cʋʋ? Mer na yɩɩraa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ teena wɩ kʋʋa'. A mɛ̃ gɩ khasa ma ciilnəə sɩ na fagʋʋ.
42023023	Sɩ wɩ bor a hulẽ jɔɔ dɩ wa-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛna aa: Kpaanɛɛ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra. Dɩ mɔna wɩ-n huleni gɩ hana gɩ ha.
42023024	Dɩ Pɩlatɩ tha thʋnɔ sa tu ayɩ, gɩrɛra wι-n bιɛlnι wι cʋɛ.
42023025	Dι a faarɛ kuunikɛ wι kɔɔ bιɛlnι, ʋrɛɛkɛ wι kɔɔ khaannι khaιra laʋna na tibil kʋrra, sa gba Jeju a ha wι mɔ̃ wι-n ƴaalnι.
42023026	Mɔna wι-n jalnanι Jeju, wι caananɛ kũu bιɛlιkɛ thɛnι lɔɔ da-n kɔ̃, a cʋgʋʋ dι heen kʋkʋ thιrʋ da-n kpana Jejura khiro. Ɔr wι-n we Sιmɔ̃, Sιrɛn a the.
42023027	Dι tιbιla jɔɔ n kɔɔ kpaaraarɛ, na khɛrasɔɔkɛ n bιɛraanι dι wa-n khιιna,
42023028	sι Jeju kιιl hιιn khɛraale sa so war: Jerujalɛm khɛra, na-n khιι mara', sι na-n khιa anι thɛthɛɛdara na anι bιsanaadara.
42023029	Nι hιnɛ, bɔɔ na daan kɛ wa sonι anayι: Gι da kʋ̃bʋʋsɔra, gι da dakha kɔ̃lʋʋsɔraakɛ na kɔnanι bi yuuə', na ilẽ bi nʋɔɔkɛ bi na kɔɔ mamιnι yuuə'.
42023030	Mɛ̃ tιbιla na ma wa-n so gɔ̃gɔ̃ kɔ̃tιnana wι yι: Nι je the sarrakɛ; na gɔ̃gɔ̃ yιrara wι yι: Nι kɛa sarrakɛ.
42023031	Gιdonι ado wι cʋʋ thale thιr huurə, anye na dana thιr khιιra?
42023032	Dι bɔ bιɛllaalera, wι kpar puu cʋʋdara yenyɔɔkɛ teananι wι kʋʋrɛ wι a kpana Jeju dakha a jalna.
42023033	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ wι danι paarιkɛ wι-n wenι Yʋ khubu, le wι kpa Jeju kʋkʋ thιrʋra nakha puu cʋʋdara yenyɔɔlera, bιɛl ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra, bιɛl ɔɔ nyɔ̃bιlana.
42023034	Sι Jeju sor: Thιrɛ, faa awι sopugo a ha wι gιdonι wa jι gιrɛɛkɛ wι-n cʋʋna'. Lιιkɛ wι kɔɔ lιnι wι tιnɛna ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ.
42023035	Dι tibil jɔɔkɛ kɔɔ hanιle jιιlɛ dι wa-n hιιn. Dι kɔ̃tιnasɔ dakha wι-n kɔɔ ɓoɓororaarɛ dι wa-n sona: Aa-n kɔɔ taa wɩ̃ tibiləə a taa ɔɔbara bɛɛ, ado ɔr dɔ Kirisitiikɛ Thãgba phiirni.
42023036	Dι sɔrasɛsɔ dakha n ɓoɓororaarɛ, a tɔ pɔ na ta ƴʋ̃ɔ dι wa-n haa sι wa-n so:
42023037	Ado fɛr dʋɔn Juifi fãgadaar, taa afιbara bɛɛ.
42023038	Dι kherereekɛ kɔɔ hanιle kʋkʋ thιrʋra ƴũ sor: Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn Juifi fãgadaar.
42023039	Dι tibil bιɛl puu cʋʋdararaakɛ wι kɔɔ kpanaanι kha kʋkʋ thιrʋra n nιιrʋʋrɛ da-n sʋʋrnaa ayι: Ga do Kirisiti fι doaa? Taa afιbara sa taa sι.
42023040	Sι ɔɔ 'walãkha bιɛl phaanʋʋnɛ ayι: Fa-n ma Thãgba gaa? Mee ga so heen ca bιɛlla fι 'lɛ dakha.
42023041	Sι ado sɛr gι, gι teere kha gιdonι sι 'lɛr gιrɛɛkɛ teananɩ asɩ cʋʋ pa. Sι ʋrɛɛkɛ, aa cʋʋ thɩ̃ puu bɩɛllaka'.
42023042	Agɩpɩ dɩ so Jejura: Jɛna mɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ fa gbanɩ fãga.
42023043	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Sobɔr mɩ so far, nĩkɛ fa har kha na mɛrɛ hɩɩr paar Thãgbaa kal ƴɔɔ.
42023044	Gɩ kɔɔ thɔɔrɛ ʋlkhɔɔ, sɩ dɩɩ koo birəre tĩtĩtĩ a dana dʋɔr bɔɔ.
42023045	Wire kɔɔ birəre, dɩ kẽkẽ nɩɩkɛ hanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna vaarɛ yenyɔ.
42023046	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ hulene nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ayɩ: Thɩrɛ, mɩ gbaar ɩ̃ thu dɩ ma-n pɛ afɩ nyɛna. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a sonɩ gele pɩ a khire.
42023047	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ yɩnɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananɩ, a-n dʋbɩrɛ Thãgbaa i ayɩ: Sobɔr gɩ, tɩɩ sarʋ kuunikɛ do ger.
42023048	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ pɔr a tor ga thɩnaale yire, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩnɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananɩ pɩ, wɩ kɛrrɛ bir dɩ wa-n kɔ̃ na ƴɛ gʋɛrɛ.
42023049	Dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ jɛnɩ Jeju na khɛrasɔɔkɛ n kɔɔ kpaaraanɩ a fʋna Galile, wɩ kɔɔ hale a jɩɩl ƴɔɔ dɩ wa-n hɩɩn gɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ.
42023050	Hɩnɛ kũu bɩɛl gɩ, a kɔɔ hale a do so gʋʋrdaar dι wa-n wιι Jojɛfι. Tιι bʋɔ gι a sarna dakha.
42023051	Aa-n kɔɔ tu ιkhasɔɔdaakɛ wι-n sona' na gιrɛɛkɛ wι-n cʋʋna'. Juifisɔɔ dιιkɛ wι-n wenι Arιmate a the. Dι a-n pιɛrɛ bɔɔkɛ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do na ιnι.
42023052	A kɔɔ ιιrɛ jal Pιlatιι pa a bιɛl a ha nι Jejuu for.
42023053	Agιpι dι gba Jejuu for a gbunə a parʋʋ kẽkẽ bulo ɓʋ̃ɔ, sa dʋʋ kaaraakɛ wι kɔɔ thelnι gɔ̃gʋɔna, kãkɛ wa kɔɔ dʋnι tibil pa'.
42023054	Sι dιι do gbɛbι wire gι, a thιɛna gaa gɛr dʋɔn hιιr wi tɔ̃tʋ̃ɔ wire.
42023055	Dι khɛrasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ thɛnι Galile nakha Jeju kɔɔ kpaanɛ Jojɛfιra a yι kaa na mɔ̃ wι dʋnι Jeju.
42023056	Dι wι kɛrrɛ bir kɔ̃ a gbɛbι niinikɛ n hʋnanι daʋ na latιkolo, sa hιιr hιιr wire mɔ̃kɛ awι jɔfʋ hanι.
42024001	Dι wire makonyɔɔ caca wi, khɛraale kɔɔ jaal kaara duuro phiphiphi na niinikɛ n hʋnanι daʋ ka, kɛ wι kɔɔ gbɛbιnι.
42024002	Dι wι yιrɛ bokaar dιι kpuro a khokhιa ka nʋɔra.
42024003	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ wι lonι wa kɔɔ yι Jeju Kɔ̃tιnι fora'.
42024004	Dι mɔ̃kɛ awι kpιɛr nyanyaanɩ, hɩnɛ kona yenyɔɔkɛ tɔnɩ kẽkenaakɛ n caranɛnɩ kɔɔ the warɛ.
42024005	Dɩ mɔ̃ maar fʋlɛ wɩnɩ ka wɩ gʋɛrɛ ƴιɛ thɩɩra, dɩ konaale bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n ƴaal ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ yidaar khee thɩ̃thɩɩn?
42024006	Aa ha ka', a ɩɩrɛ a the khirera. Sɩ nɩ jɛna mɔ̃kɛra a kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ hanɩ Galile ayɩ:
42024007	Dɔ wɩ liirna mɛr tibili Bikuun, wɩ ha sopugodara wɩ gba mɩ wɩ kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra; sɩ ma ɩɩrɛ na the khirera wire yẽther wirera.
42024008	Dɩ khɛraale jɩna Jejuu thɩmɩɩlera a kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩnɩ,
42024009	a faa kaa sa kɛr bir kɔ̃ a mɩɩ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr bɩɛl, na ɩkhasɔ fɛʋ gelela fɛʋ.
42024010	Wɩrɛ kɔɔ mɩanι ga thɩ̃ιle thɔ̃thɔna, Marιιkɛ thɛnι Magιdala gɩ, na Jan, na Marιιkɛ dʋɔnnι Jakιι nι, na wɩ̃ khɛrsɔɔkɛ wι-n kɔɔ hananι kha.
42024011	Sι thɔ̃thɔna na kɔɔ pɛ khɛraa thιmιιle haara', a gba gι dιι do war nɔ jι thιmιιr.
42024012	Dι Pιɛr ιιrɛ a ca jal kaara. Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kpuni hιιn, aa yι thɩ̃ɛ saagado kẽkẽ gborõbi haar gι dιbara gaaga, dι a faarɛ sa bir da-n kɔ̃ na nɔ kpaarɛ gιrɛraakɛra kɔɔ dananι.
42024013	Dι hιnɛ, ga wiilera kpãkpãadara yenyɔ wɛrra kɔɔ hale hʋɛra dι wa-n jal dι bιɛllaakɛ wι-n wenι Emayʋsι. Kilə yʋɔr bιɛlsɔ gι na Jerujalɛm.
42024014	Dι wa-n mιι kha gιrɛɛkɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ cʋɛnι.
42024015	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wι-n khʋɛnι kha dι wa-n bulena khasɔ, Jejuu thɛthɛ pɔr dι wι cʋr kha dι wa-n jal.
42024016	Sι gι hor thɩ̃ɛ kɔɔ yaarɛ wι dι wa jιa'.
42024017	Dι Jeju bule wi: Anye nι-n bule khasɔ dι na-n jalna? Dι wι jιιl na gbobire.
42024018	Dι bιɛl wɛrraakɛ wι-n wenι Kileopasι birsee thakɛ: Fɛr bιɛl dιbara dʋɔn kpakpalιkɛ hanι Jerujalɛm dιιra, kɛ na jɛnι gιrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananι ga wisɔraakɛra gaa ya?
42024019	Dι bule wi: Anye? Dι wι birsee: Gιrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dananι Jejuukɛ thɛnι Najarɛtι, kɛ kɔɔ dʋɔnnι Thãgbaa bobon a hana fãga thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra na thιmιιrra, Thãgbaa ƴɛra na tιbιla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra dakha,
42024020	na mɔ̃kɛ bonι jidaar kɔ̃tιna, na asι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ liirnaanι a pιɛraa so kʋnanɛ, dι wι gbaa kpa kʋkʋ thιrʋra.
42024021	Sι sι kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar ɔr na dɔra ʋrɛɛkɛ na birseneni Ɩjιraƴɛl bιsana; sι na gelesɔɔlerakɛ fɛʋ, hιnɛ, wire yẽther ha nĩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔlera kɔɔ danι.
42024022	Sobɔr gι, wɩ̃ khɛrsɔ asι thɩ̃thιιn kɔɔ mιι sɛr dι nʋɔ kpaa sι. Wι kɔɔ jaal kaara duuro phiphiphi,
42024023	sι mɔ̃kɛ wa kɔɔ yιnι ɔɔ fora', wι pɔr a mιι sι mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ kɔɔ the warnɩ a so war: A bire hana yire.
42024024	Dɩ ʋkhasɔ asɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn kɔɔ jaal kaarara dakha, a yɩ thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ ha oti mɔna khɛrasɔ kɔɔ mɩɩ sɩnɩ, sɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛ wer wa kɔɔ yɩa'.
42024025	Dɩ le Jeju so war: Pha, kũu kpɛsɛ 'leedarasɔ, gɩ-n nɩ nɛr waa sobɔr dɩ na pɛr haar gɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ sonɩ.
42024026	Ga kɔɔ teena Kirisiti n gaar bʋɔ thale sɩ a lõ ɔɔ i dʋbɩra gaa?
42024027	Agɩpɩ dɩ mɩɩ wɩ kɩrʋ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ gɩ baarɛ, a fʋna Mʋɩjɩɩ sɛbɛ a jalna gbana Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ sɛbɛ fɛʋ.
42024028	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n wɔrɔnɩ dɩɩle kãkɛ wɩ-n kɔɔ jalnɩ, Jeju cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ ho ƴɔɔ a ƴaal a kpãsɛ a jal.
42024029	Sɩ wɩ-n kɔɔ yɩrnaanɛ dɩ wa-n sʋʋraa: Birə cɔ, gɩdonɩ wire lʋʋn pɩ, dɩ dɩɩ 'li tɩɩn. Dɩ a lʋʋn wɩ cɔ kha.
42024030	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ toonɩ dɩko kho paar na wɛr, a gbaar buru a bɩɛl Thãgba pɛr. Agɩpɩ dɩ kuur a ha wɩ.
42024031	Le awɩ yi khɛr dɩ wɩ jɩɩ, sɩ dapaara a yɩrrɛ phɩɩ awɩ ƴɛra.
42024032	Dɩ wa-n mɩɩ kha awɩ ha ayɩ: Da kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na kɔɔ fʋ sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n kɔɔ mɩɩ sɩnɩ hʋɛra da-n nɩna sɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ kɩrʋaa?
42024033	Dɩ wɩ ɩɩr dapaara a kɛr bir Jerujalɛm, a yɩ yʋɔr bɩɛlɩkɛ kɔɔ gbɛbanɩ kha na awɩ kpakpaarsɔɔkɛ
42024034	kɔɔ sɔ warnɩ ayɩ: Sobɔr gɩ, Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a the khirera a nɩna ɔɔbara Sɩmɔ̃.
42024035	Dɩ le yenyɔɔle dakha kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ dana wɩnɩ hʋɛra, na mɔ̃kɛ wɩ jɩɩnɩ dabɔɔkɛ a-n kɔɔ kuurni buru.
42024036	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n mɩɩnɩ thakɛ, Jeju lʋʋn ɔɔbara awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa so war ayɩ: Nɩ hanana ha ɩɩ.
42024037	Dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ dɩ wa-n jẽ, a ka jɩna khĩdidaar wɩ yɩ.
42024038	Sɩ Jeju so warɛ: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ haar fuu ni, dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ kpɩɛr caar thakɛ ɩɩr anɩ hara?
42024039	Nɩ hɩnɛ ɩ̃ nyɛ̃ na ɩ̃ nɛ, mɛr gɩ bɔɔbɔɔ. Nɩ tha mar hɩnɛ, gɩdonɩ khĩdidaar na-n hana tomɩr dɩ khubu gɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ yɩ mɩnɩ dɩ ɩ̃ ha ga.
42024040	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ gele, a nɩna wɛr ɔɔ nyɛ̃ na ɔɔ nɛ.
42024041	Mɔ̃ daʋ kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɩnɩ wa kɔɔ pɛr haar pɩraka', dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɛr wo, dɩ Jeju bule wer: Nɩ hananɛ dɩkhaa thɩ̃ khona kɩɛr ya?
42024042	Dɩ wɩ haa thʋ̃ 'wana kur bɩɛl.
42024043	Dɩ gba a kho awɩ ƴɛra.
42024044	Agɩpɩ dɩ so war ayɩ: Gɛr dʋɔn gɩrɛɛkɛra mɩ-n kɔɔ so narnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ kha na nɛrɛ ayɩ: Dɔ gɩrɛɛkɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ kherene marnɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋra, na Thãgbaa bobonaa sɛbɛra, na Khɩkhɩɩ nɩ sɛbɛra n dã oti.
42024045	Dɩ Jeju cʋʋ awɩ kpɩɛr dɩɩ jaa war, wɩ puno wɩ jɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ kɩrʋ.
42024046	Dι a so warɛ: Mɛ̃ gɩ khere, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ teenanɛ mɛr Kirisiti n kɔɔ gaar bʋɔ sɩ ɩ̃ ɩɩr ɩ̃ the khirera wire yẽther wirera.
42024047	Dɩ ɩ̃ i wa gba na mɩɩna ha debire, na sopugo faa thɩmɩɩr tibil caarra fɛʋ, sɩ Jerujalɛm ga kɔɔ fʋ.
42024048	Nɛr dɔ sobɔ so jɩdara ga thɩnaakɛra.
42024049	Sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ mɛrɛ, ma thɔna narɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ɩ̃ Thɩ kɔɔ ʋlfɛnɩ, sɩ nɛrɛ nɩ tɔɔ kɛ dɩ bɩnɔ phaphapha nɩ 'lɛ fãgaakɛ na thɛnɩ ƴũ.
42024050	Agɩpɩ Jeju jalna wɩ a dana Betanɩ khʋra, a 'laa nyɛ̃ɛ ƴũ sa bɩɛl Thãgba a pɛ war.
42024051	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba a pɛ war a faa wɛr, sɩ dɩ Thãgba khəsuu da-n jʋʋn Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
42024052	Sɩ wɛr, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ fʋɔrʋʋnɩ pɩ, wɩ kɛrrɛ bir kɔ̃ Jerujalɛm na da kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ.
42024053	Dɩ le wɩ kɔɔ too Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna wire fɛʋ dɩ wa-n khɩɩ Thãgba.
43001001	Caca fʋ paar ʋrɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Thɩmɩɩr kɔɔ mãa hale, dɩ Thɩmɩɩrɩlera kɔɔ har kha na Thãgba, dɩ Thɩmɩɩrɩlera Thãgba a do.
43001002	Caca fʋ paar Thãgbara a hana kha.
43001003	Dɩ ɔr kɔɔ cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ cʋɛnɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ na hale a cʋʋ saagado ɔr gaaga.
43001004	Ɔrra yire n the, dɩ yireelera dɔ dahɩrɛ tɩbɩlala.
43001005	Dɩ dahɩrɛɛlera n caranɛ dabirəra sɩ dabirə na-n tegua'.
43001006	Tibil bɩɛl kɔɔ hale Thãgba thɔnɩ, ɔɔ i n dʋɔn Jã.
43001007	A ɩnɛ a do sobɔ so jɩdaar da-n mɩɩ sobɔ so jɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ dahɩrɛɛda, gɩ do nɔɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n pɛr haar.
43001008	Ga do ɔr kɔɔ dɔ dahɩra', sɩ a ɩnɛ a mɩɩ sobɔ so jɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ dahɩrɛɛda.
43001009	Dahɩrɛɛle dɔ dahɩrɛ bɔɔkɛ kɔɔ ɩnanɩ kɛ thɩɩra da-n hɩrɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
43001010	Dɩ a kɔɔ har kɛ thɩɩra dɩ ɔrra kɔɔ cʋɛ thɩɩ, sɩ tɩbɩla thɩɩra na kɔɔ jɩa'.
43001011	Ɔɔ too pa a kɔɔ ɩ̃, sɩ ɔɔ toora na kɔɔ tegua'.
43001012	Sɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ tuoneeni a pɛrna ɔɔ i haar, a-n ha wɛr punone dɩ wɩ debina a do Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔɔkɛ a-n kɔnɩ,
43001013	dɩ ga-n the thɩ kuunna ga, dɩ tibili ƴaalla ga, dɩ tibili kpɩɛr tirə ga, sɩɩ do Thãgba kɔna wɩ.
43001014	Dɩ ʋrɛra wɩ-n wenɩ Thɩmɩɩr kɔɔ debire a do tibil a toona sɩ. Dɩ sɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ dɩɩ do i dʋbɩrɛ gɩɩkɛ Bikũu bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽekɛ thɛnɩ Thɩrɛɛ pa 'lini. Sobɔdaar bire a do, dɩ bɔ jɩɩr hii bɩnɔ.
43001015	Jã kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ sobɔ so jɩɩr a pɩɛraa a hulena thakɛ ayɩ, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛra mɩ kɔɔ sonɩ ayɩ, ʋrɛɛkɛ na kpaan marnɩ, ɔr dɔ ɩ̃ ƴɛ kʋʋldaar, gɩdonɩ ɔr kɔɔ haanle sɩ dɩ ɩ̃ pɩɩrɔ.
43001016	Dɩ ɔɔ hirəra sɛrɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ 'lɛ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ na dɔnɩ dapɩnana'.
43001017	Gɩdonɩ Mʋɩjɩ Thãgba ha jɔfʋ dɩ 'laa, sɩ sobɔr na bɔ jɩɩr Jeju Kirisitira gɩ-n the.
43001018	Tibil bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ yɩ Thãgba kpɩɩraka', sɩ Bikũu bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽekɛ hanɩ Thɩrɛɛ pa, ɔr cʋɛ dɩ wɩ jɩɩ.
43001019	Nɩ yɛ Jãa sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ Juifisɔɔkɛ bonɩ jidara na wɩrɛ dɔnɩ Levɩɩ caakɛ hanɩ Jerujalɛm thɔ̃ wɩnɩ ɔɔ pa, wɩ bulenee ayɛ: Fɛrɛ, amɛ fɩ dorakɛ tɔr?
43001020	Dɩ a ture aa bana ga ayɩ: Ma do Kirisita'.
43001021	Dɩ wɩ buleele: Dɩ amɛ ha fɩ? Fɛr dɔ Elɩ Thãgbaa bobon ya? Dɩ so: Kpei ma do Elɩa'. Dɩ fɛr ba dɔ Thãgbaa bobonna yaa? Dɩ birse wi: Kpei.
43001022	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Dɩ amɛ ha fɩ? Gɩdonɩ dɔ sɩ bir sɩ so wɛkɛra thɔna sɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ. Dɩ ado fɛrra gɩ, amɛ fer yɩ fɩ dor gɩrɛ?
43001023	Dɩ so ayɩ: “Mɛr dɔ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ nʋɔɔkɛ n huleneni bəənnə ayɩ: Na-n wɛbɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋ gɩ pɔlɔ”, mɔ̃kɛ Ejaɩ Thãgbaa bobon sonɩ.
43001024	Wɩrɛɛkɛra wɩ kɔɔ thɔnɩ, jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ wɩ do.
43001025	Dɩ wɩ buleele: Dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa-n kpɛɛ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ sɩ ga do Kirisiti fɩ doa', fa do Elɩ wo, dɩ Thãgbaa bobonɩlera ga?
43001026	Dɩ Jã birse wi: Mɛrɛ, nyʋɔnɔ mɩ-n kpɛɛ tɩbɩla, sɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn bɩɛl hale na jɩna',
43001027	kɛ na kpaannɩ ɩ̃ khiro, dɩ ma hɩɩrʋʋrakɛ a na thʋbʋʋ nɛfaa pɛ̃a'.
43001028	Thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ Betanɩ gɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩr iiro ka Jana n kpɛɛnɩ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ.
43001029	A dɩɩ wɩl, Jã yɩrɛ Jeju da-n pʋɔraa dɩ so ayɩ: Nɩ yɩɛ, ɔr dɔ Thãgbaa Bana biikɛ n hɛlanɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩraa sopugo.
43001030	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛra mɩ kɔɔ sonɩ: Kũu bɩɛl hale a na kpa mar a do ɩ̃ ƴɛ kʋʋldaar, gɩdonɩ ɔr kɔɔ haanle sɩ dɩ ɩ̃ pɩɩrɔ.
43001031	Ma kɔɔ jɩa', sɩ mɔ̃ a na fʋnɩ sa a yɩr Ɩjɩrayɛldarara dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ ɩ̃ ma-n kpɛɛ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ.
43001032	Dɩ Jã mɩɩrɛ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ ayɩ: Mɩ yɩrɛ Thu Phuu dɩ the thãgbara ƴũ, a gbũ a ho puusɩ̃ɛ, a lʋʋnaa.
43001033	Ma kɔɔ jɩa', sɩ Thãgbaakɛ thɔna mɩnɩ ma-n kpɛa tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ, ɔr sɔ mar ayɩ, ʋrɛɛkɛ ma yɩnɩ Thu Phuu dɩ na gbũ na lʋʋnaa, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ na-n kpɛanɩ tɩbɩla Thu Phuurə.
43001034	Mɩ yɩ gɛr dɩ ma-n mɩɩrɔ sobɔ so jɩɩr ayɩ: Ɔr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuunna.
43001035	A dɩɩ wɩl, Jã hale dapa wo nakha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yenyɔ.
43001036	Dɩ a hɩɩnɛ Jeju n kanɩ sa bir so: Nɩ yɩɛ, ɔr dɔ Thãgbaa Bana bi.
43001037	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yenyɔɔle nɩɛrɛ gɩrɛ a sonɩ dɩ wa n kpa Jejura.
43001038	Dɩ Jeju kɩɩl a yɩ wɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa, dɩ bule wi ayɩ: Anye nɩ-n ƴaal? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Kana fɩ-n cɔ ya, Rabɩ? Rabɩ, i kɩrʋ dʋɔn Dɩɩrdaar.
43001039	Dɩ so war: Nɩ ɩna na yɩɛrɛ; dɩ wɩ jaal a yɩ kãkɛ a-n cɔnɩ. Dɩ wɩ toonaanɛ dawiile gɩdonɩ wire dʋɔrɛ.
43001040	Ãdire, Sɩmɔ̃ Pɩɛrɩ õkuun kɔɔ dʋɔn bɩɛl wɩrɛ yenyɔraakɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ Jãa thɩmɩɩkɛ a mɩɩnɩ dɩ wa-n kpaaraa.
43001041	Sɩ Ãdire dɔ cacadaarɩkɛ kɔɔ yɛnɩ Sɩmɔ̃, ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔ, a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Sɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ Mesɩ. I kɩrʋ dʋɔn Kirisiti.
43001042	Dɩ a kɔɔ kpaarɛ a jalna Jejura, dɩ Jeju hɩɩnʋʋnɛ kirkirkir sa so: Fɛr dʋɔn Sɩmɔ̃, Jãa bikuun ha fɩ, sɩ Sefasɩ wa-n we fɩ. I kɩrʋ dʋɔn Pɩɛr.
43001043	Dɩ ga dɩ wɩlla, Jeju kɔɔ ƴaalɛ a jal Galile dɩɩ do le a yɩ Filipi a sʋʋraa: Na kpa mar.
43001044	Dɩ Filipira dɩ bɩɛl a the na Ãdire na Pɩɛr, Bɛcaɩda gɩ.
43001045	Dɩ Filipi yɩrɛ Natanayɛl a sʋʋraa: Sɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ ʋrɛɛkɛra Mʋɩjɩ kherenɩ ɔɔda jɔfʋ sɛbɛra, kɛ dakha Thãgbaa bobonasɔ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ ɔɔda, kɛ dɔnɩ Najarɛtɩ Jeju, Jojɛfɩɩ bikuun.
43001046	Dɩ Natanayɛl bulee: Thɩ̃ bʋɔ na punone na the Najarɛtɩ dɩɩra ya? Dɩ Filipi sʋʋraa ayɩ: Dɩ ɩna hɩnɛ.
43001047	Dɩ Jeju yɩrɛ Natanayɛl da-n pʋɔraa, dɩ ma da-n mɩɩ ɔɔda: Nɩ yɛ kɛ Ɩjɩrayɛlda bɔɔkɛ fɩɩlɛ na harna'.
43001048	Dɩ Natanayɛl bulee: Kana fɩ jɩ mɩ? Dɩ Jeju birsee: Ɔbɔɔkɛ Filipi na kɔɔ we fɩnɩ pa', ɔbɔɔkɛ fɩ hanɩ thɩr kɩrɔ, mɩ kɔɔ mãa yɩ far.
43001049	Dɩ Natanayɛl birsee: Dɩɩrdaar, jaa fɛrra dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuunna, jaa fɛrra dʋɔn Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa fãgadaar.
43001050	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Gɩdonɩ mɩ kɔɔ so farɛ ayɩ, mɩ kɔɔ mãa yɩ far thɩr kɩrɔ, gɛr gɩ dɩ fɩ pɛr haar. Fa yɩrɛ thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩna dɩ a jɔ gɩrɛ
43001051	Dɩ Jeju bir sʋʋraa: Sobɔr mɩ so far gel, na yɩrɛ thãgbara ƴũ dɩ ga khɛrna, dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ na jʋʋnɛ sɩ wa-n gbũ mɛr tibili Bikuunna.
43002001	Wire yẽther wirera her kɔɔ har Galile Kana, dɩ Jejuu nɩ kɔɔ halera.
43002002	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ wer Jeju dakha na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara dɩ wɩ pɔ herraale.
43002003	Mɔ̃ taanɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ dɩvɛ̃ ɩnɩ dɩ ga-n ɓɔr, Jejun nɩ sʋʋraarɛ ayɩ: Wa hana dɩvɛ̃ bã.
43002004	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Khɛr, anye sɩ ha kha? Ɩ̃ bɔ na dã pa'.
43002005	Dɩ ɔɔ nɩ so thɔ̃ donana: Nɩ cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a na so narnɩ.
43002006	Sɩ boka bɩlãkpona maadõ gɩ, a kɔɔ hale dɩ wɩ thɩɩnna nyʋɔn dɩɩ do Juifisɔɔ phɔphʋɔlda. Gbõgbõ yenã dɩkha maadõ n he gɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
43002007	Dɩ Jeju so warɛ: Nɩ he bɩlãkponaakɛra nyʋɔn. Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ hi ger phi na nyʋɔnna.
43002008	Dɩ bir so war: Nɩ cɛ nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã a jalana hana dɩko tɩnɛdaar; dɩ wɩ cɛ jalna haa.
43002009	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩko tɩnɛdaar 'lɛnɩ nyʋɔnɩkɛ debanɩ a do dɩvɛ̃ hɩɩn, aa jɩ ka dɩvɛ̃ɛle thena'; sɩ thɔ̃ donaakɛ wer kɔɔ cɛnɩ nyʋɔn jɩrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ; dɩ a wer kher he,
43002010	a sʋʋraa: Dɩvɛ̃ bʋɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n 'laa caca ɓo, sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla n hini pɩ, dɩ wɩ pɩɩrɔ dɩphã gɩrɛ na jɩɛnnɩ bɔra' a na 'laa, sɩ fe wer dɩvɛ̃ bʋɔra fer thɩɩn dɩɩ ba dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ.
43002011	Galile Kana dɩɩra dɔ Jejuu caca nɔ kpaa thɔ̃ fʋ pa. Liir a nɩna ɔɔ puno hana dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara pɩɛ haar.
43002012	A gele pɩrɔ, a gbaar jal Kapɛrnayʋm na ɔɔ nɩ, na ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔsɔ, nakha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara, sɩ gbe wɩ kɔɔ too le dɩbara.
43002013	Dɩ Juifisɔɔ Pakɩ n wɔrɔnɛ, dɩ Jeju gba jal Jerujalɛm.
43002014	Dɩ a yɩrɛ le Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ tɩbɩla dɩ wa-n dolõ nasɔ, na banaasɔ, na kʋlã puosɔ, na war debidarasɔ, dɩ wɩ too dɩ wa-n debi war.
43002015	Dɩ a gbaar pɛ̃ɛ a le khasa a weelena wɩ fɛʋ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ, na banaasɔ, na nasɔra, sa gba war debaa warsɔ a jãjalã a faa, a tʋɔrna tabalsɔ a kpɛɛ,
43002016	sa so kʋlã puu dolõdarara: Nɩ thɩrɛ na gɩrɛ kɩɛr. Na-n gba ɩ̃ Thɩɩ cɔ na cʋʋ gɩ do thɩ̃ dolõ cʋɔra'.
43002017	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara jɩna dɩ gɩ kɔɔ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Afɩ cɔ thu fʋ mɛr a thʋ̃ kar.”
43002018	Dɩ Juifisɔ buleele: Anyee nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ ca fɩ-n nɩ sar dɩ fa-n cʋʋ thɩɛna thakɛ?
43002019	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Nɩ wɩɛrɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ, sɩ wire yẽther biləni ma bire na mɩɩ.
43002020	Dɩ Juifisɔ sʋʋraa: Yɛna kpalanyɔ maadõ wɩ mɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ a cʋʋna, dɩ fe wer yɩ, wire yẽther fa bire na mɩ na pɩɩ?
43002021	Sɩ jaa Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɩkɛ Jeju mɩɩnɩ kɩɛr ɔɔ tomɩ a so.
43002022	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ a the khirera, ɔɔ kpãkpãadara jɩna gɛr dɩ thalera a kɔɔ so, dɩ wɩ pɛr haar gɩrɛraakɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ na thɩmɩɩrraakɛ Jejura kɔɔ sonɩ.
43002023	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ hanɩ Jerujalɛm Pakɩ fɛtɩra, tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ pɛrɛ ɔɔ i haar, mɔ̃ wɩ yɩnɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ.
43002024	Sɩ Jeju wer na hana war ha pɛra', gɩdonɩ a jɩ wɛr fɛʋ,
43002025	dɩrakɛ aa hana ƴaalɛ tibil n mɩɛnɛ nɩ mɔ̃ tibil hana', gɩdcmɩ ɔr thɛthɛ jɩrɛ gɩrɛ n hanɩ tibili bɩnɔ.
43003001	Juifi kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl kɔɔ hale a do.lɔfu bʋ dʋdaar dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Nɩkɔdɛm.
43003002	A kɔɔ jaal Jejura dɩtɩnɔ a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Dɩɩrdaar, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ fɛr dʋɔn dɩɩrdaarɩkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa a ɩ̃, gɩdonɩ tibil na puno na cʋʋ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ ca ƴɩrɛ fɩ-n cʋʋnɩ saagado Thãgba haan kha na ntaa ga.
43003003	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Sobɔr mɩ so far gel, ado Thãgba na kɔ̃ tibil kɔ̃ phaa ga, a na puno na lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra ga.
43003004	Dɩ Nɩkɔdɛm bulee: Mɔ̃ɔ puno ca tibil na tɩ̃ na pɩ, sɩ na hana dɩ wa kʋ̃ɔ? A na punone na bir na lõ ɔɔ nɩɩ kɔ̃lora, dɩ na bir na kʋ̃ɔ balanyɔ wo ya?
43003005	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Sobɔr mɩ so far gel, ado Thãgba na kɔ̃ tibil dɩ do daphaa dɩɩ the nyʋɔnna na Thu Phuurə ga, a na puno na lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra ga.
43003006	Ʋrɛ tibil n kɔnɩ, tibillə a-n do, sɩ ʋrɛ Thu Phuu n kɔnɩ, Thu Phuudaar a-n do.
43003007	Fa-n do nʋɔ n kpaa fɩ gɩrɛraakɛ mɩ so farnɩ: Dɔ Thãgba n kɔ̃ fɩ kɔ̃ phaa ga.
43003008	Ka jɩɛ n nanɩ, le a-n phʋ̃ dɩ fɩ nɩɛ tutugore sɩ fa-n jɩ ka a thenɩ na ka a-n kana'. Thalera gɩ-n ha na tibil wo tibilikɛ Thu Phuu n kɔnɩ.
43003009	Dɩ Nɩkɔdɛm bir bulee: Mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛlera na fʋ sɩ na ha thale?
43003010	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Fɛr dɔ Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa dɩɩrdaar sɩ fa jɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkaa?
43003011	Sobɔr mɩ so far gel, gɩrɛ sɩ jɩnɩ gɛr ser n mɩɩ, dɩ gɩrɛ sɩ yɩnɩ sɩ-n mɩɩrɔ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr, sɩ na-n tu asɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩa'.
43003012	Ado na-n pɛr haar ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ mɩɩ nɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩɩda ga, mɔ̃ na pɛr haar ɔbɔɔkɛ ma mɩɩ nɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ ƴũdaa?
43003013	Tibil bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ jʋʋn Thãgbaa dʋɔ saagado ʋrɛ thɛnɩ le Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ gaaga, kɛ dɔnɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun.
43003014	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ khəini sɩ ther dɩɩ jã ƴũ bəənnə, dɔ wɩ khəi tibili Bikuun ɔmɛ̃,
43003015	dɩ mɛ̃ tibil wo tibilikɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haar ɔrra, a na hananɛ yireekɛ na pɛnɩ yuuə'.
43003016	Naʋʋkɛra Thãgba kɔɔ nanɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩra dɩɩ ka dʋɔn mɔ̃kɛ a 'laanɩ ɔɔ Bikũu bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ, dɩ mɛ̃ tibil wo tibilikɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haar ɔrra, a na bu yuuraka', sɩ a na hananɛ yireekɛ na pɛnɩ yuuə'.
43003017	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba na kɔɔ thɔ̃ ɔɔ Bikuun thɩɩraakɛ a heene tɩhɩla sora', sɩ ɔrra tɩbɩla fɛʋ na 'lɛrɔ taarɛ.
43003018	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haar ɔrra, a na 'lɛ so heena', sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haara', a 'lire 'lɛr so heene pɩ gɩdonɩ aa pɛr Thãgbaa Bikũu bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽe i haara'.
43003019	Dɩ yɛ gɩrɛ ɛnanɩ so heenena, gɛr dʋɔn dahɩrɛɛ ɩ̃ɩkɛ a ɩnɩ kɛ thɩɩra sɩ dɩ tɩbɩla na dabirə a ka jɔ dahɩrɛ, gɩdonɩ awɩ thɔ̃ puurore ka.
43003020	Gɩdonɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ puure a-n laarɛ dahɩrɛ, aa-n 'la dɩ the dahɩrɛra ga, ga hor wa yɩrɛ ɔɔ thɔ̃ɔkɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ.
43003021	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛnɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ sobɔr, ɔr n thɛ dahɩrɛra, dɩ mɛ̃ ɔɔ thɔ̃ɔkɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ n yɩr, gɩdonɩ gɩrɛra a-n cʋʋnɩ Thãgbara gɩ ha.
43003022	A gele pɩ Jeju na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara gbaar jal Jude dɩɩra, dɩ le a kɔɔ toona kpãkpãadara da-n kpɛɛ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ.
43003023	Jã dakha n kpɛɛrɛ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ Enɔ̃ɔkɛ wɔrɔnanɩ Salɩm dɩɩ, gɩdonɩ le nyʋɔn jɔr, dɩ tɩbɩla n pɔr le da-n kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔ,
43003024	gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔle wa kɔɔ fʋ Jã a to khaɩra pa'.
43003025	Sɩ Jãa kpãkpãadarasɔ nakha Juifi bɩɛl kɔɔ ɩɩrnanɛ thɩ̃ banaa phɔphʋɔl thɩmɩɩrra.
43003026	Dɩ wɩ gbaar jal Jãa pa a sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar, ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hanɩ kha na fɛrɛ Jʋrdɛ̃ iiro, kɛ fɩ kɔɔ mɩɩrɔnɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr, a hale gɩrɛ da-n kpɛɛ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ ɔɔ pa wɩ-n jal.
43003027	Dɩ Jã birse wi: Tibil na puno na 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ saagado Thãgbaa pa gɩ thaa ga.
43003028	Mee nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ dʋɔn wɩrɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ gɩrɛ mɩ kɔɔ sonɩ ayɩ: Mɛrɛ, ga do Kirisiti ha ma', sɩ thɔ̃thɔn ha mɩ ɩ̃ kʋlɛɛ ƴɩɛ a ɩna.
43003029	Dɩ ʋrɛ n hɩnanɩ khɛr, ɔr n dɔ khɛr he. Sɩ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ khɛr hee kuun n tɔɔnɩ da-n pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ nũu, daʋ n fʋʋrɛ mɔ̃ a na-n nɩɛnɩ khɛr hee wirə. Mɛ̃ gɩ daʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛda, gɩ daan waa vʋ̃ʋ.
43003030	Dɔ ɔr n kɔ̃tɩ̃ a na-n pɛr sɩ ɩ̃ tɔ ma-n wur.
43003031	Ʋrɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ, ɔr kəəne a jɔ fɛʋ; sɩ ʋrɛ wɩ kɔnɩ thɩɩra, thɩɩ tibil a do, dɩ mɔna a donɩ thɩɩ tibil mɛ̃ a-n mɩɩ thɩɩda. Ʋrɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ, ɔr kəəne a jɔ fɛʋ,
43003032	dɩ ɔr n mɩa sobɔ so jɩɩr gɩrɛraakɛ a yɩnɩ na a nɩɛna, sɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na-n tu ɔɔ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩa'.
43003033	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ tuonni ɔɔ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ, a nɩnanɛ casɩ dɩ sobɔdaar Thãgba do.
43003034	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ Thãgba thɔnɩ, thɩmɩaakɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaada a-n mɩɩ, gɩdonɩ ga do Thãgba mɩɛrɛ ɔɔ Thurə a haa ga.
43003035	Thãgba Thɩrɛ nar ɔɔ Bikuun a gba thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ a dʋʋ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
43003036	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ Bikuun haar a hananɛ yire khorr, sɩ ʋrɛ n nʋrɛnɩ nũu Bikuunna a na 'lɛ yirə', sɩ Thãgbaa nĩkhi heenuune.
43004001	Jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara nɩɛrɛ dɩ Jeju n cʋʋrɛ tɩbɩla dɩ wa-n do kpãkpãadara dɩ kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔ, dɩ wa-n.jɔ Jãa too,
43004002	sɩɩ dorakɛ ga do Jejuu thɛthɛ n kpɛa tɩbɩla nyuɔnɔa', sɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara wɛ.
43004003	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn nɩɛnɩ gelela, a faarɛ Jude dɩɩ sa ɩɩr a kɛr bir Galile.
43004004	Sɩ dɔ Jeju n the Samarɩ dɩɩra sɩ a jal.
43004005	Dɩ a kɔɔ daan Samarɩ dɩ bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Sɩsaarɩkɛ wɔrɔnanɩ lɩɛɛkɛ Jakɔbɩ kɔɔ hanɩ ɔɔ bikuun Jojɛfɩ.
43004006	Dɩ liirrə Jakɔbɩɩ bi kɔɔ ha. Sɩ mɔ̃ Jeju kɔɔ vɔɔnɩ ɔɔ kpaar pa, a toore bi nʋɔra; sɩɩ do ʋlkhɔ khʋra gɩ kɔɔ do.
43004007	Dɩ Samarɩ khɛ bɩɛl pɔ da-n cɛ nyʋɔn. Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Ha mɩ nyʋɔn ɩ̃ yɔ.
43004008	Sɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara wer kɔɔ jaal dɩɩra dɩko thɩɩ.
43004009	Dɩ Samarɩ khɛrɩle sʋʋraa ayɩ: Mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ fɛrkɛ dɔnɩ Juifi bɩɛl mɛr Samarɩdaarra nyʋɔn fɩ yɔ? Gɩdonɩ Juifisɔ na Samarɩdara na-n bɔ kha ga.
43004010	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Ado fɩ kɔɔ jɩrɛra Thãgbaa khaarda na ʋrɛɛkɛ n bɩɛlnɛ farnɩ gɩrɛ fɩ ha nɩ nyʋɔn ɩnɩ-n yɔ, ga dor fɛr na kɔɔ kara na bɩɛlaa a ha fɩ nyʋɔnɩkɛ n 'laanɛnɩ yire.
43004011	Dɩ khɛrɩle sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, fa hana thɩ̃ɛ a na cɛna ga, sɩ dɩ bire hulono. Ka fa yɩ nyʋɔnɩkɛra n 'laanɛnɩ yire?
43004012	Fɛr kɔ̃tɩna a jɔ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jakɔbɩɩkɛ kɔɔ hana sɩnɩ bireekɛra, kɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛra kɔɔ yɔnɩnakɛ na ɔɔ bikona na ɔɔ nʋ̃sɔ ya?
43004013	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Tibil wo tibilikɛ n yɔnɩ nyʋɔnɩkɛ, yɔlkhaa na fʋʋrɛ wo.
43004014	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na yɔnɩ nyʋɔnɩkɛ ma haanɩ, yɔlkhaa na fʋʋ kpɩɩ bã; sɩ nyʋɔnɩkɛ ma haanɩ ga debire na do ɔɔ bɩnɔ yɔ bu kaarɩkɛ na-n buonni gɩ haa yire khorr.
43004015	Dɩ khɛr sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ ha mɩ yɔ caakɛra dɩ yɔlkhaa na fʋ mɩ bã, dɩ ma ɩ̃ kɩɛr ɩ̃ eɛ nyʋɔn bã.
43004016	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Jala wɛ afɩ ko sa birə ɩna kɩɛr.
43004017	Dɩ khɛr sʋʋraa: Ma hana kuuna'; dɩ Jeju birsee: Sobɔr fɩ so fa hana kuuna';
43004018	gɩdonɩ kona yemɔɩ fɩ kɔɔ he, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ fɩ hananɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ, ga do afɩ ko ga, dɩ sobɔr ha gɩrɛ fɩ sonɩ.
43004019	Dɩ khɛr sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩ Thãgbaa bobon ha fɩ.
43004020	Asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ fʋɔrɛ Thãgha gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ ƴũ, sɩ dɩ ne wer n yɩ: Paarɩkɛ teananɩ Thãgba fʋɔrɛ dʋɔn Jerujalɛm.
43004021	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Khɛr pɛ mɩ haar, gɩdonɩ bɔɔ n daan, kɛ na fʋɔrnɩ Thɩrɛ gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ dɩ Jerujalɛmna gɩrakɛ woa'.
43004022	Nɛrɛ, nɩ-n fʋɔrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ na jɩna', sɩ sɛrɛ, sɩ-n fʋɔrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ sɩ jɩnɩ, gɩdonɩ Juifii caarra Taadaar the.
43004023	Sɩ bɔɔ n daan, dɩ gɩ 'lire daan pɩ, kɛ fɔfʋɔrda bɔsɔ na fʋɔrnɩ Thɩrɛ, gɩ do Thu Phuurə gɩ-n the mɔ̃ a hanɩ thʋ̃bɔr, gɩdonɩ wa fɔfʋɔrda casɔɔle Thɩrɛ n ƴaal.
43004024	Thu Phuu Thãgba do, dɩ dɔ ɔɔ fʋɔrɩkɛ wa-n fʋɔrʋʋnɩ gɩ do Thu Phuurə gɩ-n the mɔ̃kɛ a hanɩ thʋ̃bɔr.
43004025	Dɩ khɛr sʋʋraa: Mɩ jɩrɛ dɩ Mesɩ na ɩnɛ, ʋrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Kirisiti. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a na ɩnɩ a na mɩɛ sɛr thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
43004026	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Mɛrkɛra n mɩana fɩnɩ, mɛrra gɩ.
43004027	Dɩ ɔbɔɔlera ɔɔ kpãkpãadara bir pɔ dã, dɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɩ mɔna a-n mɩɩnanɩ kha khɛr. Sɩ tibil bɩɛl na-n bulelakɛ, anye a-n bule khɛrɩle, agɩbo anye a-n mɩɩnaa yaa ga.
43004028	Dɩ le khɛr faa ɔɔ yɔ cɛ da sa kɛr bir dɩɩra, a so tɩbɩlala:
43004029	Nɩ ɩna hɩnɛ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ sɔ marnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ, gɩ ba do ɔr dʋɔn Kirisitira yaa?
43004030	Dɩ wɩ ther dɩɩraale dɩ wa n pɔ Jejura.
43004031	Bɔ bɩɛllaalera kpãkpãadara n phʋʋr Jeju thakɛ ayɩ: Dɩɩrdaar, khɔ dɩkor mɛ̃.
43004032	Dɩ so war: Mɩ hananɛ dɩkorɩkɛ na jɩna'.
43004033	Dɩ kpãkpãadara na-n bule kha bɩɛlbɩɛl: Tibil ba ɩnana dɩkor a haa yaa?
43004034	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ɩ̃ dɩko dʋɔn ma-n eʋɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩɩ tuur a na cʋɛna dakha ɔɔ thɔ̃ gɩ pɩ.
43004035	Nɛrɛ, na-n so dɩ nɩ yɩ: Pora yenã sɛ wo sɩ jʋ kha bɔɔ n dã gaa? Nɩ hɩnɛ, mɩ so narɛ: Nɩ gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ a hɩnɛ jɔɔkɛ bɩnanɩ pɩ a dã kha bɔɔ.
43004036	Dɩrakɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ n khanɩ 'lire 'lɛr ɔɔ lɩmɩ pɩ, dɩ khana tɩbɩla jʋ khaa wa-n 'lɛ yire khorr, dɩ mɛ̃ ʋrɛɛkɛ n direni na ʋrɛɛkɛ n khanɩ na gbɛbɩ kha wa-n kãka.
43004037	Dɩ gɩ har mɔna wɩ-n sonɩ ger dɩ wɩ yɩ aa: Ʋ n diire dɩ ʋ n kha.
43004038	Mɩ thɔ̃ nɛr nɩ kha gɩrɛɛkɛ na kɔɔ vɔɔrɔna', ɩkhasɔ kɔɔ vɔɔ dɩ nɩ lõ awɩ thɔna.
43004039	Dɩ Samarɩdara jɔɔjɔɔ dɩɩraale kɔɔ pɛrɛ Jeju haar dɩɩ the khɛrɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩraakɛ a kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ ayɩ, a so narɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ɩnɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ.
43004040	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Samarɩdara pɔnɩ a yɩɩ, wɩ bɩɛlʋʋlɛ a tɔɔna nɩ kha, dɩ Jeju toona wɛr wire yenyɔ.
43004041	Dɩ Samarɩda jɔjʋɔ bir jɩɩ pɛr haar wo dɩɩ do Jejuu thɩmɩɩ dɔ nɔɔ,
43004042	sɩ dɩ wa-n so khɛrraale: Ga do gɩrɛɛkɛ fɩ mɩɩ sɩnɩ gɛr cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sɩ pɛr haar bã, sɩ gɩdonɩ sɩ nɩɛrɛ asɩbara a jɩ dɩ ɔr dʋɔn tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩraa Taadaar sobɔr.
43004043	A wire yenyɔɔle ka pɩ, Jeju ther le da-n jal Galile.
43004044	Gɩdonɩ Jejuu thɛthɛ kɔɔ sor ayɩ: Thãgbaa bobon bɩɛl na-n 'lɛ cʋrɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ dʋɔa'.
43004045	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju danɩ Galile, Galiledara teguure gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a kɔɔ cʋunɩ Jerujalɛm fɛtɩ bɔɔ. Gɩdonɩ wɛr dakha kɔɔ jaal fɛtɩraale.
43004046	Dɩ Jeju kɛr bir Galile Kana, kãkɛ a kɔɔ debini nyʋɔn dɩɩ do dɩvɛ̃. Dɩ fãgadaarɩ thɔ̃daar kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl gɩ, a hale Kapɛrnayʋm dɩ ga-n kho ɔɔ bikuun.
43004047	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a nɩɛnɩ dɩ Jeju ther Jude a bir ɩ̃ Galile, a jaalaalɛ a bɩɛlʋʋ a pɔ a kpɛɛnɛ ɩnɩ bikuunikɛ gɩ-n khonɩ, dɩɩ sɩ gbe sɩ a ɓɔr.
43004048	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa ayɩ: Ado na-n yɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔa', na-n pɛr haar kpɩɩraka'.
43004049	Dɩ fãgadaarɩ thɔ̃daar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, ɩna ɓo sɩ ɩ̃ bɩsã na ɓɔr na pa'.
43004050	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Kɔna, afɩ bikuun na khə'. Dɩ kuunile pɛrɛ thɩmɩɩrɩle Jeju sʋʋraanɩ haar, a gba jal da-n kɔ̃.
43004051	Dɩ mɔ̃ a 'lini gba hʋɛ pɩ da-n kɔ̃, ɔɔ thɔ̃dara caanʋʋnɛ hʋɛra a sʋʋraa: Afɩ bɩsã kpɛɛrɛ.
43004052	Dɩ bule wi: Ʋmɔ̃ bɔra gɩ kɔɔ baaraanɩ? Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: De gɩ wire n ganɩ gbe, gɛr tomɩ kporre ɩɩraa.
43004053	Dɩ le thɩrɛ jɩ dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛra Jeju kɔɔ sʋʋraanɩ ayɩ, ɔɔ bikuun kpɛɛrɛ wa bɔɔlera gɩ, dɩ ɔr na ɔɔ cɔdara fɛʋ pɛr haar.
43004054	Gɛr dʋɔn balanyɔ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ Jeju cʋʋnɩ wo, ɔbɔɔkɛ a thenɩ Jude a kɛr bir Galile.
43005001	A gele pɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ hananɛ fɛtɩ Jerujalɛm, dɩ Jeju jal.
43005002	Dɩɩraale yɔ hulẽ paar hale a wɔrɔna Bana lookɛ wɩ-n wenɩ na ebirə thɩmɩɩr Bɛtɛsɩda, dɩ paar yemɔɩɩkɛ hɔnɩ jɛ̃bɛrɛ̃ kɔɔ harɔrɛ.
43005003	Dɩ paarɩkɛ hɔnɩ jɛ̃bɛrɛ̃ɛle khodara jɔɔ n kɔɔ phɩnɛ le, yarasɔ, nɛ kʋɛdarasɔ, gbãgbarasɔ, [kɛ n tɔɔnɩ le dɩ wa-n pɩɛr yɔ tutugore,
43005004	gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu n gbune dɩkhãa bɔɔ yɔ hulẽ paarɩle da-n tutugo nyʋɔn. Dɩ khodaarɩkɛ n kɔɔ gbunoni caca ɔbɔɔkɛ nyʋɔn n tutugoni, ado ɔɔ kho ha mɔnakɛ sɩ gɩ-n kpɛɛrɛ.]
43005005	Dɩ kũu bɩɛl kɔɔ hale dɩ khoo fʋʋ dɩ cʋʋna yɛna kpelẽ yʋɔr makõther.
43005006	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju yɩɩnɩ dɩ phɩ̃, a jɩrɛ dɩ khoo kɔɔ fʋʋrɛ a maan kɛkɛkɛ, sɩ a buleele ayɩ: Fɩ-n ƴaalɛ fɩ kpɛɛ khoora ya?
43005007	Dɩ khodaarra birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, ma hana tibilikɛ na gbaan mɩnɩ na thɩɩn ka nyʋɔn n tutugonə', gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ma-n jalnɩ tɩɩ kpɩɩ n kɔɔ kʋʋl mɛr ƴɩɛ dɩ gbũ.
43005008	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Ɩrɛ gba afɩ jɔ̃ a kɔna.
43005009	Dɩ dapaara kuunile kpɛɛ a ɩɩr gba ɔɔ jɔ̃ a jal da-n kɔ̃. Sɩ hɩɩr wire wireele kɔɔ do.
43005010	Dɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ bulele kuunile kpɛɛnɛnɩ: Fɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do hɩɩr wire gɩ, dɩ fa hana hʋɛ na heen afɩ jɔ̃a'.
43005011	Dɩ birse wi: Ʋrɛɛkɛ kpɛɛnɛ mɩnɩ ɔr sɔ mar ayɩ, ɩ̃ gba ɩ̃ jɔ̃ a kɔna.
43005012	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Amɛ wer dɔ kuunilera sɔ farnɩ fɩ gba afɩ jɔna a jala?
43005013	Sɩ kuunile khoo kpɛɛnɩ na kɔɔ jɩ ntɛ kpɛɛnɛɛna', gɩdonɩ Jeju lʋʋn tibil jɔraale kɔɔ hanɩ paarɩle.
43005014	Dɩ a gele pɩ, Jeju yɩɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna a sʋʋraa: Fɩ jɩrɛ fɩ kpɛɛrɛ gɩrɛ. Fa-n bir cʋʋ sopugo dɩ dɩkhaa puukɛ jɔnɩ gɩrɛ n bir gɩ dã fɩ bã.
43005015	Dɩ kuunile jaal a so Juifisɔra: Jeju gɩɩkɛ kɔɔ kpɛɛnɛ mɩnɩ.
43005016	Gɛr hɩna waa dɩ Juifisɔ ma dɩ wa-n kpoo Jejura, gɩdonɩ hɩɩr wire a kɔɔ cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔle.
43005017	Sɩ Jeju so warɛ: Ɩ̃ Thɩ n dor thɔma a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ, dɩ mɛrɛ dakha na-n do oti.
43005018	Sɩ mɔ̃ a sonɩ thale waa, gɛr Juifisɔ bir dɩ wa-n jɩɩ ƴaal wɩ kʋʋ, gɩdonɩ ga do hɩɩr wireele a cʋʋnɩ thɔma dɔ kɩrʋ dɩbara ga, sɩ gɩdonɩ a sor ayɩ, Thãgba dɔ ɩnɩ Thɩ bɩnɔ aa, ɩnɩ ha pa na Thãgba bɩɛlla gɩ.
43005019	Sɩ Jeju birse wer: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ga do mɛr Bikuun hana punone dɩ ma-n cʋʋna thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ ɩ̃bara ga. Gɩrɛ mɩ-n yɩnɩ Thɩrɛ dɩ cʋʋna, gɛr mɩ-n cʋʋ dɩbara. Gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thɩrɛ n cʋʋnɩ, gɛr mɛr Bikuun n cʋʋ oti.
43005020	Gɩdonɩ Thɩrɛ n nar mɛr Bikuun dɩ nɩ mar gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ɔr thɛthɛ n cʋʋnɩ. Sɩ a na nɩ marɛ thɔ̃ kɔ̃tɩna dɩ ma cʋʋ dɩ ga jɔ gɩrɛ wo, dɩ mɛ̃ nʋɔ na kpaa nɩ dɩphã waa.
43005021	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ Thɩrɛ n ɩɩrnɩ khe khirera dɩ ha wɩ yire, mɛ̃ mɛr Bikuun na 'laa yire na ha ʋrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n pɛrnɩ haar ɩ̃ ha.
43005022	Thɩrɛ na do tɩbɩlaa Kɩɩldaara', sɩ mɛr Bikuun a ha punone fɛʋ ɩ̃ dɔ tɩbɩlaa Kɩɩldaar,
43005023	dɩ mɛ̃ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na cʋ mɛr Bikuun, mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n cʋnɩ Thɩrɛ. Ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n cʋɔnnɩ mɛr Bikuuna', aa-n cʋ dakha Thɩrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩna'.
43005024	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ʋrɛɛkɛ n pɛnɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ nũu dɩ pɛrna haar ʋrɛraakɛ thɔna mɩnɩ, a hananɛ yire khorr. A na 'lɛ so heena', sɩ a ther khirrə a lõ yirera.
43005025	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, bɔɔ n daan dɩ gɩ 'lire daannakɛ pɩ, kɛ khe na nɩnɩ mɛr Thãgbaa Bikuuni nɔ, dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ na nɩɛnɛnɩ na bire na hana yire.
43005026	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ Thɩrɛɛ thɛthɛ donɩ Yi hɩ̃daar, mɛ̃ dakha a ha mɛr Bikuun punone dɩ ɩ̃ do Yi hɩ̃daar.
43005027	A har mɛr Bikuun hʋɛ dɩ ma do tɩbɩlaa Kɩɩldaar dakha, gɩdonɩ tibili Bikuun mɩ do.
43005028	Na-n do nʋɔ n kpaa nɩ gelela ga, gɩdonɩ bɔɔ n daan dɩ khe fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ kaʋ na nɩrɛ ɩ̃ nɔ a na ɩɩr na the.
43005029	Wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ bɔɔ na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera na 'lɛ yire khorr, sɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ puure na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera a na 'lɛ so heene.
43005030	Mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na hana punone a na cʋʋna thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ ɩ̃bara ga. Mɔ̃ mɩ nɩɛnɩ Thɩrɛɛ nɔra, mɛ̃ mɩ-n kɩɩlna tɩbɩla, dɩ ɩ̃ kɩɩl sarrɛ gɩdonɩ ga do ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ tuur mɩ-n cʋa', sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩɩ tuur mɩ-n cʋʋ.
43005031	Ado mɛr mɩa sobɔ so jɩɩrɩkɛ dɩ ma-n pɛ ɩ̃barara, ɩ̃ sobɔ so jɩ na do sobɔra'.
43005032	Sɩ ʋkha hale kɛ mɩanɩ sobɔ so jɩɩr a pɛ mɛrɛra, dɩ mɩ jɩrɛ dɩ ɔɔ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ a mɩɩnɩ a pɛ mɛrɛra dor sobɔr.
43005033	Nɛrɛ, nɩ kɔɔ thʋɔn tɩbɩla Jãa pa dɩ mɩɩ sobɔ so jɩɩr da-n pɛ sobɔrra.
43005034	Sɩ mɛrɛ, ga do tibili sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ mɩ-n ƴaala', sɩ mɩ sor gelela nɩ 'lɛ taarɛ.
43005035	Jã kɔɔ hʋrɛ lãphãakɛ n hɩrɛnɛnɩ, dɩ nɩ kɔɔ ture dɩ na-n kãka bɔɔ gbe ɔɔ hɩrɛra.
43005036	Sɩ mɛrɛ mɩ hananɛ sobɔ so jɩɩrɩkɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ a jɔ Jãada, gɩdonɩ thɔmaakɛ Thɩrɛ ha mɩnɩ ɩ̃ cʋɛ dɩ ma-n cʋʋ, gɛr n nɛna sobɔ so jɩɩr mɛrɛra dɩ Thɩrɛ thɔna mɩ.
43005037	Dɩ Thɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ thɔna mɩnɩ,.ɔɔ thɛthɛ n mɩa sobɔ so jɩɩr mɛrɛra. Na kɔɔ nɩ ɔɔ nɔ kpɩɩraka', dɩ na kɔɔ yɩ dakha ɔɔ ƴɛbi kpɩɩa'.
43005038	Dɩ ɔɔ so na too nɛrɛra ga, gɩdonɩ na-n pɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ a thɔnɩ haara'.
43005039	Nɩ-n hɩɩnɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ dɩ na-n kpãkpaanɔ, gɩdonɩ nɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ le na 'lɛ yire khorr, dɩ gɛr thɛthɛra n mɩa sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr mɛrɛra.
43005040	Sɩrakɛ na-n ƴaal nɩ ɩ̃ mar nɩ jɩɩ 'lɛ yirə'.
43005041	Ga do tɩbɩlala mɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ i dʋba'.
43005042	Sɩ mɩ jɩ nɛr: Na-n na Thãgba na haara'.
43005043	Ɩ̃ Thɩɩ i mɩ ɩna sɩ na-n tee ma', sɩ a tɩɩ kpɩɩ ka gba ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ dɩbara i a ɩna, ɔr nɩ-n ka tee.
43005044	Mɔ̃ na puno na pɛr haar nɛrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ n thɛnɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛlɩ pa, sɩ dɩ nɩ ka bo na-n ƴaal i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa dɩbara ga.
43005045	Na-n kpɩɛr dɩ mɛr na pɛ nar sor Thɩrɛɛ ƴɛra ga. Sɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ thɛthɛɛkɛra nɩ hananɔnɩ nũ pɛrɛ, ɔr na pɛ nar sor.
43005046	Ado nɩ kɔɔ pɛr Mʋɩjɩ haar gel, na kɔɔ pɛ mɛr haar dakha gɩdonɩ ɩ̃da a kɔɔ khere.
43005047	Sɩ ado na-n pɛr haar gɩrɛ a kherena', mɔ̃ na fʋ sɩ na pɛr ɩ thɩmɩɩ haar?
43006001	A gele pɩ Jeju jaal Galile mɩɩr nɔ iiro, kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ dakha Tɩbɛrɩadɩ mɩɩr nɔɔ.
43006002	Dɩ tɩbɩla jɔɔ kpaaraarɛ, gɩdonɩ wɩ yɩrɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ khodarara.
43006003	Dɩ Jeju jʋʋn gɔ̃gʋɔna a too le nakha ɔɔ kpãkpãadara.
43006004	Sɩ Pakɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Juifisɔɔ fɛtɩ kɔɔ wɔrɔnɛ.
43006005	Dɩ Jeju na-n hɩɩn a yɩ tibil jɔ dɩ wa-n pʋɔraa, dɩ bule Filipi: Ka sa yɩ dɩkɔ na the na ha tɩbɩla fɛʋʋkɛ?
43006006	Sɩ a buleele thale a hɩɩn a jɩ mɔ̃ Filipi na tuni, gɩdonɩ ɔr Jejuu thɛthɛ jɩrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ a na cʋʋnɩ.
43006007	Dɩ Filipi birsee: Ado sɩ gbarakɛ wire taanyɔ thɔ̃ lɩmɩnɛɛ war a thena buru fɩɩfɩɩ sa tɩnɛ wɩ, sɩrakɛ ga taa wɩ bʋɔa'.
43006008	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadaar bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Ãdireekɛ dɔnɩ Sɩmɔ̃ Pɩɛrɩ õkuun sʋʋraa:
43006009	Kũubir hakɛ na buru yemɔɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ bɔdaardaa na thʋma yenyɔ, sɩ anye gɩrɛ na cʋʋ tibil jɔ thakɛ tə̃tə̃tə̃?
43006010	Dɩ Jeju so: Nɩ cʋɛ tɩbɩlaalera wɩ too; sɩ hʋɔn kɔɔ jɔrɛ dapaale. Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ too, sɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan kona gbɩlanɩ yemɔɩ.
43006011	Dɩ Jeju gba buruulera. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ fʋɔrnɩ Thãgba pɛr pɩ, a tɩnɛnɛ welela tɔɔnɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ a tɩnɛ wɩ dakha thʋma mɔ̃ wɩ-n ƴaalnɩ.
43006012	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ khonɩ fɛʋ a hi phi, Jeju sor ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara: Nɩ ule dakuruukɛ nɩ tɩnɛnɩ sa sɩ na-n faa gɩ kʋɛa'.
43006013	Dɩ wɩ uule a hi kpona yʋɔr yenyɔ bɔdaar buru yemɔɩɩlera wɩ tɩnɛ wɩnɩ, dɩ wɩ kho a hi sɩ dɩɩ sɩ.
43006014	Tɩbɩlaakɛ yɛnɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ Jeju cʋʋnɩ, wɩ sor: Sobɔr gɩ, ɔr dɔ Thãgbaa bobonɩlera, kɛ ɩnanɩ thɩɩra.
43006015	Dɩ Jejn jɩrɛ dɩɩ do wa pɔr na tii na fãga, wɩ pɛr a do fãgadaar; gɛr gɩ dɩ bir faa wɩ wo sa ɩɩr dɩbara a jal gɔ̃gʋɔna.
43006016	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ birəni, Jejuu kpãkpãadara gbune mɩɩr nʋɔra,
43006017	a lõ gboroona a phɛl wa-n jal Kapɛrnayʋm khʋra. Sɩ dɩɩ do dɩɩ 'lire tɩɩn sɩ Jeju na caan wɩ pa'.
43006018	Dɩ jɩɛ kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ na fãga dɩ nyʋɔn na-n ubiri.
43006019	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ phɛllɛ a dana kilə yemɔɩ agɩbo maadõsɔ, sɩ na jɩ a yɩ Jeju dɩ ɩɩr nyʋɔnna ƴũ da-n pɔ a wɔrɔ̃ gborõo, dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ.
43006020	Sɩ Jeju so war: Mɛr gɩ, na-n do maar n fʋ na'.
43006021	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛla a lona gboroona, sɩ dɩɩ do dapaara gborõo thʋrɛ ka wɩ-n jalnɩ.
43006022	A dɩɩ wɩl tɩbɩlaakɛ kɔɔ sɛnɩ gɩ̃ iiro kɔɔ yɩɛrɛ dɩ gborõ bɩɛl sɛ le dɩbara, dɩ Jeju na kɔɔ lõ gboroonaale na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara ga, sɩ kpãkpãadara dɩbara kɔɔ jala.
43006023	Sɩ yɛ̃ gborõsɔɔkɛ kɔɔ ther Tɩbɛrɩadɩ a pɔ jɩɩl khunə, ka Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ fuɔrnɩ Tbagba a pɛ burura sɩ dɩ wɩ kho.
43006024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil jɔɔle yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do Jeju na hale dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara wa', wɩ kɔɔ luun gborõosɔraale dɩ wa-n jal Kapɛrnayʋm Jejuu ƴaal pa.
43006025	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil jɔɔle kɔɔ danɩ gɩ̃ mɩɩr nɔ iiro a yɩ Jeju, wɩ buleele: Dɩɩrdaar ya, ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ fɩ dã kɩɛr?
43006026	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, dɩkɔɔkɛ nɩ khonɩ a hi gɛr nɩ-n ƴaal mar gɩrɛ wer, ga do nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ gɛrra ga.
43006027	Na-n do thɔma dɩkorraakɛ n kʋɛana', sɩ na-n dɔ thɔma dɩkorraakɛ na punoneni a na 'laa yire khorr, dɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun na hana nɩ dɩko caalera, gɩdonɩ Thãgba Thɩrɛ ha mɛr ɔɔ puno.
43006028	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ bulee: Dɩ anye sa cʋʋ gɩrɛ kper gɩ do gɛr dɔ thɔmaakɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ?
43006029	Dɩ Jeju so war: Thɔmaakɛ Thãgba n ƴaal narnɩ dʋɔn nɩ pɩɛr ʋrɛɛkɛ a thɔnɩ haar.
43006030	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Anyee nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ ca fɩ cʋʋ dɩ sɩ yɩɛ a na pɛ fɩ haar? Anye dɔ thɔmaakɛ fɩ-n cʋʋnɩ?
43006031	Asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ khor maan bəənnə, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “A kɔɔ ha wɛr buruukɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ dɩ wɩ kho.”
43006032	Dɩ Jeju so war: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ga do Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ hana nɩ buruukɛ kɔɔ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔa', sɩ ɩ̃ Thɩ n hana nɩ buru bɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
43006033	Gɩdonɩ buruukɛ Thãgba 'laanɩ dɔ ʋrɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, a gbũ da-n 'laa yire tɩbɩlala fɛʋ thɩɩra.
43006034	Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ na hana sɩ ga buru caale wire wire.
43006035	Dɩ Jeju so war: Mɛr dʋɔn buruukɛ n 'laanɛnɩ yire; ʋrɛɛkɛ n ɩna marnɩ kɔmɛr na fʋʋ yuuə', dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ pɛ mɩnɩ haar yɔlkhaa na fʋʋ kpɩɩ bã.
43006036	Sɩ mɩ kɔɔ so narɛ ayɩ: Nɩ kɔɔ yɩ mɛr sɩ na-n pɛ haara'.
43006037	Wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thɩrɛ n ha mɩnɩ na-n ɩ̃ marɛ, dɩ ma bo ʋrɛ n ɩna marnɩ na faa kpɩɩraka'.
43006038	Gɩdonɩ mɩ ther Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ thɩɩra, ga do mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ cʋʋ ɩ̃ tuurə', sɩ mɩ ɩnɛ ɩ̃ eʋʋ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩɩ tuur.
43006039	Dɩ nɩ hɩnɛ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩɩ tuurrə dʋɔn: Ma-n faa wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a ha mɩnɩ bɩɛl n buə', sɩ ɩ̃ cʋɛ wɩ wɩ ɩɩr wɩ the khirera pɩpɩɩ wire.
43006040	Nɩ yɛ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Thɩrɛɛ tuur wo: Gɛr dʋɔn tibil wo tibilikɛ n yɛnɩ Bikuun dɩ pɩɛ haar, a-n hananɛ yire khorr, dɩ ma cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ na ɩɩr na the khirera pɩpɩɩ wire.
43006041	Sɩ Juifisɔ mar dɩ wa-n hũhuun gɩrɛraakɛ Jeju sonɩ ayɩ, ɩnɛr dʋɔn buruukɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ.
43006042	Dɩ wɩ so: Jeju, ga do Jõjɛfɩɩ bikuun a doaa? Sɩ jɩrɛ ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ, sɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ dɩ so ayɩ, Thãgbaa dʋɔ ɩnɩ the a gbũ?
43006043	Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɩ sɛro hũhuuneekɛra nɩ-n hũhuunni kha.
43006044	Tibil bɩɛl na hale na puno na ɩ̃ mar saagado Thɩrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ halaa gaaga'. Sɩ ma cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ a na the khirera pɩpɩɩ wirera.
43006045	Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ khera thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ ayɩ: “Thãgba na dɩrɛ wɩ fɛʋ.” Tibil wo tibilikɛ n pɛnɩ Thɩrɛ nũu da-n 'lɛna ɔɔ dɩɩr n ɩ̃ marɛ.
43006046	Ga do mɩ sonɩ thale waa mɩ yɩ tibil kɔɔ yɩrɛ Thɩra', ʋrɛ dɩbara thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa, ɔr yɛ Thɩrɛ.
43006047	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ʋrɛɛkɛ pɛ mɩnɩ haar, a hananɛ yire khorr.
43006048	Mɛr dʋɔn buruukɛ n 'laanɛnɩ yire.
43006049	Anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ khor maan bəənnə sɩ wɩ khiire.
43006050	Sɩ buruukɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ dʋɔn buruukɛ tibil na khonɩ a na khi kpɩɩa'.
43006051	Mɛr dʋɔn buruukɛ dɔnɩ yireekɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ. Ado tibil kho buru caakɛra, a na hananɛ yire khorr; dɩ buruukɛra ma 'laanɩ ɩ̃ tomɩ gɩɩkɛ ma 'laanɩ, dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩra na 'lɛrɔ yire.
43006052	Dɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ ɩɩrnanɛ thɩ̃ banaa awɩ ha dɩ wa-n so: Mɔ̃ kuunikɛ na puno na ha sɩ ɔɔ tomɩ dɩ sa kho?
43006053	Dɩ Jeju so war: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ado na kho mɛr tibili Bikuuni toma', dɩ a na yɔ mɛr tibili Bikuuni tɔmã', nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na puno na hana yire anɩbara ga.
43006054	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n khɔnɩ ɩ̃ tomɩ da-n yɔna ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃, a hananɛ yire khorr, dɩ ma ɩɩrʋʋrɛ khirera pɩpɩɩ wire.
43006055	Gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ tomɩ dʋɔn dɩko bɔ gel, dɩ ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃ dʋɔn thɩ̃ yɔna bɔ gel.
43006056	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n khɔnɩ ɩ̃ tomɩ da-n yɔna ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃ n toore mɛrɛra, dɩ ɩ̃ haaraa dakha.
43006057	Mɔ̃kɛ Thɩrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ dɔnɩ yidaar, dɩɩ do dakha yireekɛ mɩ hananɩ Thɩrɛɛ pa gɩ the, mɛ̃ dakha ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n khɔ mɩnɩ na hana yireekɛ na thɛnɩ mɛrɛra.
43006058	Nɩ yɛ buruukɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ a gbũ, ga ho gɩrɛ anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ khonɩ sa khiirə'. Ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n khɔnɩ buruukɛ a na hananɛ yire khorr.
43006059	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla Kapɛrnayʋm Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra, gɛr a mɩɩrɔ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ.
43006060	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla kɔɔ pɛnɩ Jeju nũu pɩ, ɔɔ kpãkpãadara jɔɔjɔɔ sor aa: Thɩmɩɩ ca gɩrɛ khɩɩrɛ kpɛ. Amɛ na punone na pɛ nũu?
43006061	Mɔ̃ Jeju jɩnɩ dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara n hũhuune kha gelelala, gɛr gɩ dɩ bule wi: Gelela do narɛ nɛ baradaa ya?
43006062	Dɩ anye na so dɩphã, ado na yɩ mɛr tibili Bikuun dɩ ma jʋʋnna ka mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ mamara?
43006063	Thu Phuu n 'laanɛ yire, tibil na-n puno gele dɩ cʋa'. Thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ, Thu Phuudaa gɩ dɩ ga-n 'laa yire.
43006064	Sɩ dɩ ɩkhasɔ nɛrɛra na-n pɛr haara'. Gɩdonɩ Jeju kɔɔ mãa jɩrɛ kɛkɛkɛrakɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ na-n pɩɛrnɩ haara', na ʋrɛɛkɛ na lirenaanɩ.
43006065	Sɩ a bire so wo: Gɛr gɩ mɩ kɔɔ so narɛ ayɩ: Tibil bɩɛl na puno na ɩ̃ mar saagado Thãgba hana ntɛ hʋɛaa ga.
43006066	A fʋna ɔbɔɔlera waa ɔɔ kpãkpãadara bərəəm kɛrrɛ bir sa fagʋʋ, wa-n kpaaraa bã.
43006067	Dɩ Jeju bule ɔɔ kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔ ayɩ: Sɩ nɛrɛ dakha na-n ƴaal nɩ jala ya?
43006068	Dɩ Sɩmɔ̃ Pɩɛr birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, amɛra sa jal? Fɛr hɩna thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ n 'laanɛnɩ yire khorr.
43006069	Dɩ sɛrɛ, dɩ sɩ pɛr haar nɛnɛ̃ a jɩ dɩɩ do fɛr dʋɔn Tɩɩ phuukɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa.
43006070	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ga do mɛr kɔɔ phire nɛr yʋɔr yenyɔaa? Sɩrakɛ tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra dor kɔ̃tɛɛbuu.
43006071	Judasɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Sɩmɔ̃ɔ bikuun, kɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ a so. Gɩdonɩ Judasɩ dorrakɛ tibil bɩɛl kpãkpãadara yʋɔr yenyɔra, sɩɩ do ɔr na lirena Jeju.
43007001	A gele pɩ Jeju n kɔɔ kpaarɛ Galile; aa kɔɔ ƴaal a kpaar Judea', gɩdonɩ Juifisɔ n ƴaalɛ hʋɛ wɩ kʋʋ.
43007002	Mɔ̃kɛ Juifisɔɔ fɛtɩɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Wa fɛtɩ n danɩ,
43007003	Jejuu õkũu bɩnɔsɔ sʋʋraarɛ aa: Thɛ kɩɛr a jala Jude, dɩ mɛ̃ afɩ kpãkpãadara na yɩ dakha thɔmaakɛ fɩ-n cʋʋnɩ.
43007004	Ado tibil ƴaal wɩ jɩɛnɛɛ, aa-n ker gɩrɛɛkɛ a-n cʋʋna'. Ado fɩ-n cʋʋrɛ thɔmaakɛ gel, cʋɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n yɩ fɩ.
43007005	Gɩdonɩ ɔɔ õkũu bɩnɔsɔ dakharakɛ na-n pɩɛ haara'.
43007006	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ɩ̃ bɔ na dã pa', sɩ ne wer, anɩ bɔ n daan bɔɔ fɛʋ.
43007007	Tɩbɩla thɩɩra na puno na laar na', sɩ mɛr wɩ-n laar gɩdonɩ easɩ mer n mɩɩ dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ, awɩ thɔ̃ puurore ka.
43007008	Nɩ jala fɛtɩraale anɩ ha. Me wer ma jal ga fɛtɩraala', gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ bɔ na jɩɩ dã pa'.
43007009	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a so warnɩ gele pɩ, a toore Galile.
43007010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jejuu õkũu bɩnɔsɔ kɔɔ jalnɩ fɛtɩraale pɩ, a kpaanɛ dakha, sɩ a wolone gɩdonɩ aa ƴaal tɩbɩla n ja'.
43007011	Dɩ Juifisɔ na-n ƴaalʋʋ le fɛtɩraalera dɩ wa-n so: Ka kuunna ba ha ya fɛ?
43007012	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle n hũhuune kha ɔɔdara dɩ wɛ n yɩ: Tɩɩ bʋɔ gɩ; wɛ n yɩ: Kpei, a-n fɩɩlɛ tɩbɩla.
43007013	Sɩ tɩbɩla na-n cã dɩ wɩ mɩɩ ɔɔda ga, gɩdonɩ maar n fɔ wɩ Juifisɔra.
43007014	Mɔ̃ wɩ-n cʋʋnɩ fɛtɩ a ha thɩ̃thɩɩn, gɛr Jeju jaal Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna a ma da-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ.
43007015	Dɩ nʋɔ kpaa Juifisɔ dɩ wa-n so: Mɔ̃ kuunikɛ fʋ sa jɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ thakɛ, aa kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ sɛba?
43007016	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Dɩɩrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla ga the ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ pa ga, sɩ Thãgbaakɛ thɔna mɩnɩɩ pa gɩ the.
43007017	Ado tibil ƴaalɛ a cʋʋ Thãgbaa tuur, a na jɩrɛ ado dɩɩrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla Thãgbaa pa gɩ the, agɩbo ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ pa ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ the.
43007018	Tibilikɛ n mɩanɩ thɩmɩaakɛ thɛnɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ pa, ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ i a-n ƴaal, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔnaanɩɩ i n dʋbarɔ, sobɔdaar a do, fɩl gõgolõ na haaraa ga.
43007019	Mʋɩjɩ na kɔɔ ha nɩ jɔfʋaa? Sɩ tibil bɩɛl anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩnnakɛ na kɔɔ nɩ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ nũə'. Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n ƴaal hʋɛ nɩ kʋ mɩ?
43007020	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle birsee: Kɔ̃tɛɛbuu ha farɛ. Amɛ n ƴaalɛ fɩ yʋʋ?
43007021	Dɩ Jeju birse wer: Thɩ̃ bɩɛl dɩbara mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ sɩ dɩ nʋɔ kpaa nɩ fɛʋ.
43007022	Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ ha nɛr jɔfʋ nɩ kuro bɩsana khʋ̃ʋ, sɩrakɛ ga do Mʋɩjɩɩ thɛthɛɛ pa jɔfʋʋlera tha', sɩ anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ pa gɩ the, dɩ nɩ-n kurre tibil khʋ̃ʋ hɩɩr wire.
43007023	Dɩ mɔ̃ nɩ-n kurni tibil khʋ̃ʋ hɩɩr wire dɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ na-n kʋɛa', mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nĩkhii n fʋ nɩ mɛrɛra gɩrɛraakɛ mɩ kpɛɛnɩ kũu bɩɛl khoo fɛʋ hɩɩr wire?
43007024	Na-n kɔɔ jɩ gɩ na yinə a 'laa na yɩ tibili da', sɩ nɩ dɔ gɩ hana hʋɛ sɩ na-n so.
43007025	Dɩ wɩ̃ Jerujalɛmdara n sor ayɩ: Ga do ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ wɩ-n kɔɔ ƴaalnɩna wɩ kʋaa?
43007026	Nɩ yɛ mɔ̃ a-n mɩɩnɩ dɩphã casɩ, sɩ wa-n cʋgʋʋ thɩ̃a'. Asɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ jɩrɛ gel dɩ ɔr dʋɔn Kirisiti bɛ?
43007027	Sɩ ado Kirisiti na ɩ̃, tibil na jɩ kana a na thena', sɩ ʋrɛ sɩ jɩrɛ ka a thenɩ.
43007028	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, gɛr a huleno ayɩ: Nɩ jɩ mɛr, dɩ nɩ jɩrɛ dakha ka mɩ thenɩ. Sɩ nɩ jɛ, ga do mɛr jɛ gɩ dɩbara a ɩ̃a', sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ sobɔdaar gɩ sɩ na jɩa'.
43007029	Sɩ mɛrɛ, mɩ jɩɩrɛ gɩdonɩ ɔɔ̃ pa mɩ the dɩ ɔr thɔna mɩ.
43007030	Dɩ le wɩ kɔɔ ƴaal wɩ fʋʋra, sɩ tibil na thaaraa nyɔ̃a', gɩdonɩ ɔɔ bɔ na kɔɔ dã pa'.
43007031	Sɩ jɔjʋɔ tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thɩɩn kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ haar, sɩ dɩ wa-n so: Ɔbɔɔkɛ Kirisiti na ɩnɩ, a na cʋʋrɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ na jɔ kuunikɛ woo?
43007032	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ tibil jɔ n hũhuunni Jejuu sora. Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara kɔɔ thʋɔn gardɛ wɩ fʋɔnɛɛ.
43007033	Dɩ Jeju so: Mɩ har kha na nɛrɛ wo gɩ dana bɔɔ gbe, sɩ ɩ̃ jal ʋrɛraakɛ thɔna mɩnɩ.
43007034	Na ƴaal mɛr sɩ na yɩ ma', dɩ ka ma hanɩ na puno na pɔa'.
43007035	Dɩ Juifisɔ na-n mɩɩ kha awɩ ha ayɩ: Kana a na jal dɩ sa puno na yɩa ya fɛ? Juifisɔraakɛ bɩ̃bɩlanɛnɩ a ha Gɩrɛkɩsɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn a na ba jal a na-n dɩɩr Gɩrɛkɩsɔ ya?
43007036	Anye dɔ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛɛ kɩr a sonɩ: Na ƴaal mɛr sɩ na yɩ ma', dɩ wo, na puno na pɔ ka mɩ hana'.
43007037	Fɛtɩɩ pɩpɩɩ wiikɛ dɔnɩ wi kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, dawiilera Jeju ɩɩr tɩbɩlaa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn a hulẽ ayɩ, ado yɔlkhaa fʋ tibil, a pɔ ɩnɛrɛra a yɔ.
43007038	Ʋrɛɛkɛ pɛ nɩnɩ haar, mɩɩr yɔ yire na celle ɔɔ bɩnɔ ga-n the mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ.
43007039	Thu Phuukɛ tɩbɩla na pɛrnɩ haar na 'lɛ, gɛr Jeju mɩɩ; gɩdonɩ Thãgba na kɔɔ 'laa Thu Phɩm pa', gɩdonɩ Jeju na kɔɔ bir jʋʋn ɔɔ Thɩɩ dʋɔ pa'.
43007040	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil ɩkha tibil jɔraale nɩnɩ ga thɩmɩɩsɔɔle pɩ, wɩ sor: Thãgbaa bobonɩlera kuunikɛ do waa gel.
43007041	Dɩ ɩkhasɔ so: Kirisiti gɩ; dɩ ɩkhasɔ n yɩ: Mɔ̃ ga fʋ sɩ dɩ Kirisiti na the Galile?
43007042	Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: Davɩdɩɩ məllə Kirisiti na the Bɛtɩlɛhɛm dɩɩra, ka Davɩdɩ kɔɔ hanɩ.
43007043	Dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ tibil jɔɔle kɔɔ lee kha Jejuu sora.
43007044	Dɩ ɩkhasɔ wɛrra kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ fʋʋ, sɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ thaaraa nyɔ̃a'.
43007045	Dɩ gardɛsɔ kɛrrɛ bir bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔɔ pa, dɩ wɩ bule wi: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na fʋʋ ɩna ga?
43007046	Dɩ gardɛsɔ birse wi: Tibil bɩɛl na kɔɔ mɩɩ thɩmɩɩr kpɩɩrakɛ kuuni khaakɛ pa'.
43007047	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara bir bule wi: Dɩ nɛrɛ dakha, wɩ fɩɩl nɛr wo koe?
43007048	Asɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, agɩbo jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ bɩɛl ʋkha kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ haar ya?
43007049	Sɩ tibil jɔɔle na jɛnɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋa', wɛr dɔ tɩbɩlaakɛ wɩ sonɩ nʋɔ pɛ.
43007050	Nɩkɔdɛmɩkɛ dɔnɩ bɩɛl jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarara hale, kɛ kɔɔ jalanɩ mamara a yɩ Jeju, a bule wer:
43007051	Ado asɩ jɔfʋra gɩ, hʋɛ hale dɩ sa heen tibil sor ɓo, sɩ sɩ pɩɩrɔ sɩ nɩɛ na asɩ nũ gɩrɛ a sonɩ sɩ jɩna gɩrɛ a cʋʋnɩ ya?
43007052	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Fɛrɛ dakha, Galile fɩ the ya? Jɩɛ 'lo Thãgbaa sɛbɛ a hɩnɛ, fa yɩɛ dɩ ga so kpɩɩrakɛ nayɩ: Thãgbaa bobon bɩɛllakɛ na the Galile dɩɩra ga.
43007053	[Agɩpɩ wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl bɩlanɛ a kɔ̃ awɩ cɔnanɔ.
43008001	Sɩ Jeju gba jal gɔ̃gʋɔnaakɛ hananɩ olɩvɩ thɩra.
43008002	A dɩɩ wɩl duuro phiphiphi, a kɛrrɛ bir Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ gbɛbɩ a pʋɔraa, dɩ too sa ma da-n dɩɩr wɩ.
43008003	Dɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdarasɔ na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kpa khɛrɩkɛ wɩ fʋnɩ dɩ phɩna kuun a pɔna. Dɩ wɩ cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ too tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra,
43008004	sɩ dɩ wɩ so Jejura: Dɩɩrdaar, kuun khɛrɩkɛ phɩna dɩ wɩ fʋʋ.
43008005	Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋra gɩ so sarɛ sɩ dʋrɛ khɛr thakɛ na bokana a kɔ. Sɩ ado fɛrra gɩ, mɔ̃ fɩ-n so?
43008006	Sɩ wɩ sor thale a benaa bɩnɛ wa-n hɩɩn, gɩdonɩ hʋɛ wɩ-n ƴaal wɩ pɩɛraa sor. Sɩ Jeju gʋɛrɛ da-n khere kherere thɩɩra na nyɔ̃bire.
43008007	Sɩ mɔ̃ wɩ bonɩ dɩ wa-n bulee, Jeju gbaar ƴɩɛ ƴũ sa so war: Ntɛɛkɛ na kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ sopugo kpɩɩrakɛ nɛrɛra ga n dɔ cacadaar a dʋɔ na bokaar.
43008008	Sɩ a bire a gʋɛ wo da-n khere kherere thɩɩra.
43008009	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ thɩmɩɩ caale, wɩ mar dɩ wa-n thɩɩr bɩɛlbɩɛl, kɔ̃tɩnasɔ kɔɔ ɩrɛ ɓo dɩ pɩpɩra na-n kpaan. Agɩpɩ Jeju sɩ dɩbara na khɛrɩle dɩ jɩɩl ɔɔ ƴɛra.
43008010	Dɩ Jeju bir gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ sa bulee: Khɛr ya, dɩ ka afɩ so pɛdarasɔra ha? Tibil bɩɛl na kɔɔ heen fɩ soraa?
43008011	Dɩ khɛr birsee: Kpei Kɔ̃tɩn. Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Dɩ mɛrɛ dakha, ma heen fɩ sora'. Jala kɔna, sɩ a fʋna nĩ fa-n bir cʋʋ sopugo kpɩɩ bã.]
43008012	Jeju bire mɩɩna wɩ wo ayɩ: Mɛr dʋɔn dahɩrɛ tɩbɩlala thɩɩra. Ʋrɛɛkɛ n kpaan marnɩ a na ɩɩr dabirəra kpɩɩraka', sɩ a na hananɛ dahɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ yireeda.
43008013	Dɩ liirrə jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ sʋʋraa: Fɩ-n mɩɩrɛ afɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ dɩ fa-n pɛ afɩbara, afɩ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ na do sobɔra'.
43008014	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ado ma mɩɩrakɛ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr a na pɛ ɩ̃bararakɛ, sɩ ɩ̃ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ dʋɔn sobɔr, gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩrɛ kãkɛ mɩ thenɩ a ɩ̃, na kãkɛ mɩ-n jalnɩ. Sɩ nɛrɛ, na jɩ kãkɛ mɩ thena' na kãkɛ mɩ-n jalna'.
43008015	Nɛrɛ, nɛr dɔ kɩɩldaraakɛ n kɩlɛnɩ mɔ̃kɛ tibil fɩlɛ hanɩ, sɩ mɛrɛ, ma do tɩbɩlaa Kɩɩldaara'.
43008016	Sɩ ado mɩ dor tɩbɩlaa Kɩɩldaar, ɩ̃ kɩɩl dor sobɔr gɩdonɩ ma ha dɩbara ga, sɩ Thɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ thɔna mɩnɩ sɩ hana kha.
43008017	Anɩ jɔfʋra gɩ kherere ayɩ: Tɩbɩla yenyɔɔ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩ dʋɔn sobɔr.
43008018	Mɩ-n mɩɩrɛ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr dɩ nɩa-n pɛ ɩ̃bara, dɩ Thɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ thɔna mɩnɩ a-n mɩɩrɛ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩrra da-n pɛ mar wo.
43008019	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Kana afɩ thɩ ha? Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Na jɩ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ Thɩ gɩ dɩ na ja'. Ado nɩ kɔɔ jɩ mɛr, na jɩrɛ ɩ̃ Thɩ dakha.
43008020	Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ ga thɩmɩɩsɔɔle, ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n dɩɩr wɩnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, kãkɛ wɩ-n pɛrnɩ Thãgba mũsumo, sɩ tibil bɩɛl na kɔɔ fʋʋa', gɩdonɩ ɔɔ bɔ na kɔɔ dã pa'.
43008021	Dɩ Jeju so warɛ wo ayɩ: Mɩ-n jaal sɩ na ƴaal mɛr, dɩ na khiire anɩ sopugorara. Na puno na pɔ kãkɛ mɩ-n jalna'.
43008022	Dɩ Juifisɔ na-n so: Dɩbara a na ba kʋ yaa, gɩdonɩ a sor ayɩ, sa puno na pɔ kãkɛ ɩnɩ-n jalna'.
43008023	Dɩ so war: Nɛrɛ, tɩɛrdara nɩ do, sɩ mɛrɛ dɩ ɩ̃ do ƴũdaar. Nɛrɛ, nɩ dor thɩɩkɛɛda, sɩ mɛrɛ ma do thɩɩkɛɛda ga.
43008024	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ so nar: Na khiire anɩ sopugosɔrara. Gɩdonɩ ado na-n pɛr haar dɩ mɛr dʋɔna', na khiire anɩ sopugosɔrara.
43008025	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Amɛ fɩ do? Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Mɔ̃kɛra mɩ kɔɔ so narnɩ caca fʋ paar gɩ.
43008026	Mɩ hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ bərəəm anɩdara a na so sɩ na kɩɩlna nɩ. Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ dʋɔn sobɔdaar, dɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ mɩ kɔɔ nɩɛraanɩ gɛr mɩ-n so tɩbɩlala.
43008027	Sɩ wa kɔɔ jɩrakɛ dɩ Thɩrɛɛda a-n mɩɩ wa'.
43008028	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ɔbɔɔkɛ na khəini mɛr tibili Bikuun, le na jɩrakɛ dɩ mɩ dor dɩ ma-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ ɩ̃bara ga, sɩ mɩ-n mɩɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ Thɩrɛ kɔɔ dɩɩr mɩnɩ.
43008029	Ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩ, a har kha na mɛrɛ. Aa faa mɩ dɩbara ga, gɩdonɩ wire fɛʋ mɩ-n eʋʋ gɩrɛ n daaraanɩ.
43008030	Mɔna a-n mɩɩnɩ thale tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ haar.
43008031	Dɩ Jeju so Juifisɔraakɛ kɔɔ pɩɛnɩ haar ayɩ: Ado nɩ too ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩra, na dor ɩ̃ kpãkpãadara sobɔr,
43008032	dɩ na jɩrɛ sobɔr, dɩ sobɔrra na cʋʋ nɛr dɩ na do waɩa.
43008033	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Abɩrahamɩ məl sɩ do, sa kɔɔ do tibili dee kpɩɩraka', sɩ mɔ̃ fɩ so aa, sa debire a na do waɩa?
43008034	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, tibil wo tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ sopugo, sopugoo dee a do.
43008035	Dee na-n too cʋɔrɔ khorra', sɩ ado bikuun gɩ, ɔr n tɔɔ cʋɔrɔ khorr.
43008036	Ado Bikuun birsene ni ga dor waɩa nɩ do waa gel.
43008037	Mɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do Abɩrahamɩ məl ha nɩ, sɩ dɩ na-n ƴaal nɩ kʋ mɩ, gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ na yɩ lõ paar anɩ hara ga.
43008038	Me wer, gɩrɛɛkɛ mɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩra gɛr mɩ-n mɩɩ. Sɩ nɛrɛ, nɩ-n cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ anɩ thɩra.
43008039	Dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Abɩraham dʋɔn asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃. Dɩ Jeju so war: Ado nɩ dor Abɩrahamɩ bɩsãsɔ, na-n cʋɛ Abɩrahamɩ thɔ̃.
43008040	Nɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɛnɛ̃kɛ nɩ kʋ mɩ mɛrkɛ sɔ narnɩ sobɔrɩkɛ mɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ Thãgbara. Abɩraham na kɔɔ cʋʋ gela'.
43008041	Anɩ thɩɩ thɔ̃ nɩ-n cʋʋ. Dɩ wɩ birsee: Sa do khɛr pɔɩ bɩsãsɔa', Thɩ bɩɛl dɩbara sɩ hana Thãgba gɩ.
43008042	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ado Thãgba kɔɔ dʋɔn anɩ Thɩ na-n na mɛr, gɩdonɩ Thãgbara mɩ the a ɩ̃. Ga do mɛr jɛ gɩ a ɩ̃ ɩ̃bara ga, sɩ ɔr kɔɔ thɔna mɩ.
43008043	Mɔ̃gɩdo na-n jɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔ kɩrʋa? Gɩdonɩ na puno na pɛ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ nũə'.
43008044	Satã dʋɔn anɩ thɩ, dɩ nɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛɛkɛ anɩ thɩ tuni. Tɩɩ kʋdaar a kɔɔ dorakɛ caca fʋ paar, dɩ aa-n jɩɩl sobɔrra ga, gɩdonɩ sobɔr na haaraa kpɩɩa'. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n kurni sõsor, ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ fɛʋ ɔɔ thɛthɛra gɩ-n the, gɩdonɩ sõsodaar a do na sõsorɩ thɩ.
43008045	Sɩ mɛrɛ gɩdonɩ sobɔr mɩ-n so, gɛr gɩ na-n pɛ mɩ haara'.
43008046	Amɛ nɛrɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn na nɛ marrakɛ sopugookɛ mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ? Dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo, ado mɩ so nar sobɔrrakɛ, na-n pɛ mɩ haara?
43008047	Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Thãgbaada, a-n pɛr Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ nũu. Nɛrɛ, na-n pɛ nũə' gɩdonɩ na do Thãgbaada ga.
43008048	Dɩ Juifisɔ bule Jeju: Sa hana hʋɛ a na so nayɩ, fɛr dʋɔn Samarɩdaar dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbuu ha faraa ya?
43008049	Dɩ Jeju so war: Kɔ̃tɛɛbuu na ha mara', sɩ ɩ̃ Thɩ mɩ-n cʋ. Sɩ nɛrɛ, na-n cʋ ma'.
43008050	Ma-n ƴaal ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ i dʋba', sɩ bɩɛl hale da-n ƴaal gɩ sa do Kɩɩldaar.
43008051	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, tibilikɛ n hɩnɛnɩ ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ, a na khi kpɩɩraka'.
43008052	Dɩ Juifisɔ sʋʋraa: Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã, sɩ jɩrɛ mɛ̃ dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbuu ha farɛ. Abɩraham kɔɔ khire na Thãgbaa bobonasɔ dakha, sɩ fɛrɛ dɩ fɩ so: Ado tibil na hɩɩn afɩ thɩmɩɩ a na khi kpɩɩraka'.
43008053	Fɩ ba kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ n dɔnɩ Abɩrahamɩkɛ khenɩ yaa? Thãgbaa bobonasɔ dakha khiire; sɩ fɛrɛ, amɛ fɩ-n pɛr haar fɩ dor?
43008054	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ado ma dʋbɩ ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ i, ɩ̃ i dʋbɩ na do thɩ̃a'. Sɩ ɩ̃ Thɩ gɩɩkɛ n dʋbanɩ ɩ̃ i, dɩ ɔrra nɩ-n so dɩ nɩ yɩ, ɔr dʋɔn anɩ Thãgba.
43008055	Sɩ na jɩɩraka', sɩ me wer, mɩ jɩɩrɛ. Ado mɩ kɔɔ sor ayɩ ma jɩa', gɩ hʋrɛ mɩ dor sõsodaar anɩ kha. Sɩ mɩ jɩɩrɛ dɩ ma-n hɩɩnna ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ.
43008056	Daʋ kɔɔ fʋrɛ anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abɩraham da-n kãka, gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ hananɛ ha pɛrɛ ɩnɩ-n yɛ ɩ̃ Wi. Dɩ a kɔɔ yɩɛrɛ dɩ daʋ fʋʋ.
43008057	Dɩ Juifisɔ sʋʋraa: Mɔ̃ fɩ cʋʋ sa yɩ Abɩraham, fa hananɩ yɛna kpalanyɔ yʋɔr pa?
43008058	Dɩ Jeju so war: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, Abɩraham na kɔɔ thenɩ dɩɩrarakɛ pa', mɛrɛ mɩ dor.
43008059	Dɩ liir dɩphã mɛ̃ wɩ uul bokana wɩ dʋʋrʋʋ, sɩ dɩ Jeju wolõ the Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ.
43009001	Mɔ̃ Jeju n kanɩ na hʋɛ, a yɩrɛ kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ kɔnɩ na yaarɛ.
43009002	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara bulee: Dɩɩrdaar, amɛ kɔɔ cʋɛ sopugo dɩ wɩ kʋ̃ɔ na yaarɛ, ɔr gɩ yaa, ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ gɩ?
43009003	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ga do ɔr ga, dɩ ga do wo ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ kɔɔ cʋɛ sopugoə', sɩ Thãgba n nɩna ɔɔ thɔ̃ ɔrra.
43009004	Dɔ sɩ do ʋrɛɛkɛ thɔna mɩnɩɩ thɔ̃ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ hanɩ gɩrɛ dɩwɩlʋla. Dɩɩ n tɩnɛ kɛ tibil na punoni a na do thɔma bã.
43009005	Mɩ dor dahɩrɛ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ thɩɩra bɔɔkɛ mɩ hanɩ thɩɩra.
43009006	Mɔ̃ a sonɩ thale pɩ, a phiire nyɔ̃thɩ̃ɩ thɩɩra a dʋ jaar na ɔɔ nyɔ̃thɩna. Agɩpɩ dɩ gba jaarɩlera a bʋl yaarʋ yinə,
43009007	sɩ a sʋʋraa: Jala hɔ nyʋɔn Siloe yɔ hulẽ paar. Siloe kɩrʋ dʋɔn thɔnanɛ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a jalnɩ a hʋ nyʋɔn pɩ sa kɛr da-n bir, a-n yɩrɛ.
43009008	Dɩ ɔɔ cɔ khʋdara nakha wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ jɩɛnɛɛnɩ mamara dɩ dona bɛ̃bɩɛl n sor aa: Ga do kɩɛr ʋrɛɛkɛ n kɔɔ too sɩ da-n bɩɛl thɩ̃aa?
43009009	Dɩ ɩkhasɔ sor: Ɔr gɩ; sɩ ɩkhasɔ wo sor: Kpeehe, ɔr ga, sɩ wɩ-n hʋrɛ kha. Sɩ dɩ yaarʋʋ thɛthɛ so war ayɩ: Mɛr gɩ sobɔr.
43009010	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ afɩ yisɔ khɛr?
43009011	Dɩ birse wi: Kuunikɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jeju, ɔr kɔɔ do jaar a bʋl mɩ yinə sa so mar: Jala hɔ nyʋɔn Siloe yɔ hulẽ paar. Dɩ ɩ̃ jal a hʋ nyʋɔn, dɩ ma-n yɩ.
43009012	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Ka kuunilera ha? Dɩ birse wi: Ma ja'.
43009013	Dɩ wɩ kpa kuunikɛra kɔɔ dɔnɩ yaarʋ a jalna jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔɔ pa.
43009014	Sɩ hɩɩr wire Jeju kɔɔ dʋ jaarra a khɛrnaa yinə.
43009015	Gɛr gɩ dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ dakha bule kuunile mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ sɩ dɩ ɔɔ yisɔ khɛr da-n yɩ. Dɩ birse wi: Jaar a bʋl mɩ yinə sɩ dɩ ɩ̃ hʋ nyʋɔn, dɩ ma-n yɩ.
43009016	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩkhaa jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kɔɔ so: Kuunikɛ dɔnɩ thɔ̃ caakɛ ga do Thãgbaa pa a tha', gɩdonɩ aa-n hɩɩn hɩɩr wirə'. Dɩ ɩkhasɔ kɔɔ sor dakha wo: Mɔ̃ tibilikɛ dɔnɩ sopugodaar na puno a na cʋʋ ga nɔ kpaa thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ? Dɩ liir dɔ leereekɛ ɩrɛnɩ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
43009017	Dɩ wɩ bir bule wo ʋrɛɛkɛra kɔɔ yaarɛnɩ ayɩ: Sɩ fɛrɛ, anye fɩ-n so ɔɔdara gɩrɛraakɛ a khɛr fɩnɩ yinə? Dɩ birse wi: Thãgbaa bobon gɩ.
43009018	Sɩ Juifisɔ na kɔɔ pɛr haar kpɩɩrakɛ dɩ a kɔɔ dor yaarʋ sa bir da-n ya', phaphapha dɩɩ dana bɔɔkɛ wɩ wenɩ ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ,
43009019	a bule wi: Ʋrɛ dʋɔn anɩ bikuunikɛra nɩ sonɩ ayɩ, nɩ kʋɔnɛ na yaarɛɛ? Dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ da-n yɩ nɛnɛ̃?
43009020	Dɩ ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ birse wi: Sɩ jɩrɛ wer asɩ bikuun gɩ dɩ sɩ kɔnaa yaarɛ.
43009021	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ a-n yɩnɩ nɛnɛ̃, sa jɩ gera', dɩ ntɛɛkɛ khɛraanɩ yinə dakha wo, sa jɩa'. Nɩ bulenee, a daan a mɩɩ dɩbara gɩrɛ baannɩ.
43009022	Ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ sor thale gɩdonɩ maar fɔ wɩ Juifisɔra, gɩdonɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ 'lire gʋʋrɛ kha nɔ bɩɛl ayɩ: Ado tibil tu ayɩ, Jeju dor Kirisiti, wa tiire awɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra a na faa.
43009023	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɔɔ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ kɔɔ so ayɩ, a daan a mɩɩ dɩbara wɩ bulenee.
43009024	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara bir a we kuunikɛ kɔɔ dɔnɩ yaarʋ wo a sʋʋraa: Dʋba Thãgbaa i. Sɛrɛ, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sopugodaar kuunikɛ do.
43009025	Dɩ birse wi: Ado sopugodaar a do, ma jɩ gera', sɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛlɩkɛ mɩ jɩnɩ dʋɔn: Mɩ kɔɔ dor yaarʋ, sɩ nɛnɛ̃ mɩ-n yɩrɛ.
43009026	Dɩ wɩ bulee: Mɔ̃ a khɛr fɩ yinə, dɩ anye a cʋʋ fɩ?
43009027	Dɩ birse wi: Mɩ kɔɔ mãa so nar sɩ na kɔɔ pɛ nũə'. Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nɩ bir na-n ƴaal nɩ nɩɛ wo? Nɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɩ debi nɩ do ɔɔ kpãkpãadara dakha yaa?
43009028	Dɩ wɩ nɩɩrʋʋ sa sʋʋraa: Fɛr dʋɔn ɔɔ kpãkpãadaar, se wer Mʋɩjɩɩ kpãkpãadara ha sɩ.
43009029	Dɩ ado Mʋɩjɩ gɩ, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ mɩanaa, sɩ ado ʋrɛɛkɛ gɩ sa jɩ kãkɛ a thena'.
43009030	Dɩ kuunile birse wi: Pha, nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ gɩ na jɩ kãkɛ a thena', sɩ a khɛr mɛr yinə.
43009031	Sɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do Thãgba na-n tu sopugodaraa bɩɛla', sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n maannɩ Thãgba da-n cʋʋna Thãgbaa tuur, ɔ tibil caalee bɩɛl Thãgba n tu.
43009032	Dɩ wo sa kɔɔ nɩɛ kpɩɩrakɛ dɩ wɩ mɩɩna ayɩ, tibil bɩɛl kɔɔ khɛrrɛ yaarʋʋkɛ wɩ kɔnanɩ yaarɛ yinə ga.
43009033	Ado kuunikɛ na kɔɔ the Thãgbaa pa ga, a na puno na cuu thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ kpɩɩa'.
43009034	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Fɛrkɛ wɩ kɔnɩ sopugo haarra, fɛr n ka dɩɩr sɩ bɛɛ? Agɩpɩ dɩ wɩ weguu.
43009035	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ wɩ weguure a faa, a ƴaalʋʋlɛ a yɩɩ a bulee: Fɩ pɛr tibili Bikuun haar bɛ?
43009036	Dɩ bule Jeju: Amɛ a do ya Kɔ̃tɩn dɩ ma pɩɛ haar?
43009037	Dɩ Jeju birsee: Fɩ yɩɩrɛ, ʋrɛɛkɛra n mɩana fɩnɩ ɔr gɩ.
43009038	Dɩ tu: Kɔ̃tɩn, mɩ pɛrɛ haar; sa gburõku da-n fʋɔrʋʋ.
43009039	Agɩpɩ Jeju so: Kɩɩlʋ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ ɩnɔ thɩɩraakɛ, dɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ na-n yɛna' wa-n yɩrɛ, sɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ n yɛnɩ wa debire na do yara.
43009040	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ hananɩ kha Jeju, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ thɩmɩaale pɩ, wɩ buleele: Dɩ sɛrɛ, yarara sɩ do dakha gaa bɛ?
43009041	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Ado yara nɩ kɔɔ do, na hana sopugoə', sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ dɩ nɩ so: Sɩ-n yɩrɛ; gɛr gɩ dɩ anɩ sopugo dakha hale 'lo.
43010001	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n lonanɩ bana cʋɔr na lõfonʋɔa' sɩ dɩ lona pa kpɩɩ, tibil ca ole dʋɔn yu na yu hɔ̃hʋɔldaar.
43010002	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ lonananɩ lõfonʋɔ, ɔr dʋɔn bana khedaar.
43010003	Lo hɩɩndaar na khɛrʋʋrɛ loo, dɩ banaa na nɩɛrɛ ɔɔ nɔ. Dɩ a na wer banaasɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔda awɩ i bɩɛlbɩɛlbɩɛl a cʋʋ wɩ wɩ thɩɩr jɩɛra.
43010004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a na tini banaasɔ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔda na pɩ, a na kʋʋl wɛr ƴɩɛ wa-n kpaaraa, gɩdonɩ wɩ jɩrɛ ɔɔ nɔ.
43010005	Wa kpa kpakpalla ga, wa fagʋʋrɛ sɩ na ca gɩdonɩ wa jɩ kpakpalaa nɔa'.
43010006	Jeju so warɛ sokpaakɛ, sɩ wa jɩrakɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ a ƴaalnɩ a so wara'.
43010007	Dɩ Jeju bir so war wo ayɩ: Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, mɛr dʋɔn bana loo.
43010008	Wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ kʋlɛ mɩnɩ ƴɩɛ a ɩ̃ dʋɔn yo na yu hɔ̃hʋɔldara, sɩ banaa na kɔɔ pɛ wɩ nũə'.
43010009	Mɛr dʋɔn lõfonʋɔ. Ntɛɛkɛ na lona marnɩ a na 'lɛr taarɛ. A na lʋʋn a na the sɩ a na yɩrɛ dɩkor.
43010010	Yu na ɩ̃ sɩɩ do aa yuə', sɩɩ do aa kʋa', sɩɩ do aa kʋɛaa ga. Sɩ mɛrɛ, mɩ ɩnɛ banaa n hanana yire dɩ wa hana gɛr dɩ ga jɩɩ jɔr.
43010011	Mɛr dʋɔn bana khedaar bʋɔ. Dɩ bana khedaar bʋɔ n faarɛ ɔɔ yi banaa sora.
43010012	Sɩ bana hɩɩndaarɩkɛ na dɔnɩ bana khedaara', dɩ ʋrɛ hɩnanɩ banaa ga, ado a yɩ kpe da pɔ a-n faarɛ banaa sɩ dɩ ca; dɩ kpe n pɔ dɩ fʋlɛ wɩ sɩ dɩ bɩ̃bɩlã wɩ.
43010013	A-n car gɩdonɩ warra a-n do ɔɔ thɔ̃, sɩ aa-n therna banaa ga.
43010014	Mɛr dʋɔn bana khedaar bʋɔ. Mɩ jɩrɛ ɩ̃ banasɔ dɩ ɩ̃ banasɔ jɩ mɛr dakha,
43010015	mɔ̃kɛ Thɩrɛ jɩ mɩnɩ dɩ ɩ̃ jɩ Thɩrɛ. Dɩ mɩ faarɛ ɩ̃ yi banaa sora.
43010016	Mɩ hananɛ bana kpɩɩsɔ wo, kɛ na-n lonanɩ nakha ɩ̃ banaakɛ cɔ bɩɛlla'. Wɛr dakha mɩ teenanɛ ɩ̃ kpa wɩ a ɛna. Dɩ wa nɩɛrɛ ɩ̃ nɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ wa do bana ca bɩɛl wɩ hana bana khedaar bɩɛl dakha.
43010017	Thɩrɛ n na mɛr gɩdonɩ mɩ faarɛ ɩ̃ yi sɩ ɩ̃ bir ɩ̃ gba.
43010018	Tibil bɩɛl na tee mar ɩ̃ yiika', sɩ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ faa gɩ dɩbara. Mɩ hananɛ punone a na faana, dɩ mɩ hananɛ punone a na gbana gɩ. Gɛr dʋɔn hʋɛɛkɛ mɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩra.
43010019	Dɩ ga thɩmɩɩsɔɔlera ɩrɛna leere wo Juifisɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
43010020	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn na-n so ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɛɛbuu hanaanɛ, dɩ yʋʋ kʋɛsʋʋ. Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n pɛ ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ nũu?
43010021	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ bor sa so war: Ga do kɔ̃tɛɛbuda thɩmɩa ha gɩra'. Kɔ̃tɛɛbuu na punone a na khɛr yarasɔ yinə ya?
43010022	Ɔbɔɔlera yʋʋrɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ phʋɔl fɛtɩ ha Jerujalɛm.
43010023	Dɩ Jeju na-n kpaar Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna paarɩkɛ hɔnɩ jɛ̃bɛrɛ̃ɛkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Salomɔ̃ɔda.
43010024	Dɩ Juifisɔ kpa jɛ a diirəə sa bulee: Ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ ga thʋ̃ na dã sɩ dɩ fa ti si baalɛɛkɛ n ha sɩnɩ haarra wire wo wire? Ado fɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti, sɔ sar casɩ.
43010025	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Mɩ kɔɔ so narɛrakɛ sɩ na-n pɛr haara'. Thɔmaakɛ mɩ-n gbanɩ ɩ̃ Thɩɩ i dɩ ma-n cʋʋna, gɛr n nɛna sobɔ so jɩɩr mɛrɛra.
43010026	Sɩ nɛrɛ, na-n pɛr haara' gɩdonɩ na do ɩ̃ banasɔa'.
43010027	Ɩ̃ banasɔ n nɩrɛ ɩ̃ nɔ, dɩ mɩ jɩ wɛr dɩ wɩ-n kpa marɛ;
43010028	dɩ mɩ ha wɛr yire khorr, dɩ wa bu yuuraka', dɩ tibil gɩ a və̃ wi a taa ɩ̃ nyɔ̃kɔa'.
43010029	Ɩ̃ Thɩɩkɛ hana mɩnɩ a kəəre thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, dɩ tibil bɩɛl na hale a na puno na və̃ wi ɩ̃ Thɩɩ nyɔ̃kɔa'.
43010030	Dɩ mɛrɛ na Thɩrɛ bɩɛl sɩ do.
43010031	Dɩ gɛrra gɩ dɩ Juifisɔ bir uul bokana wo wɩ dʋʋrnaa.
43010032	Dɩ Jeju bir so war wo ayɩ: Mer eʋʋ nɩnɩ dɩ nɩ jɩ ɩhɔ̃ bɔ jɔjʋɔsɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Thɩrɛra, gɩmɔna nɩ-n dʋʋrna mɩ bokana?
43010033	Dɩ Juifisɔ birsee: Sa n dʋʋrna fɩ bokana thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋ thɩmɩɩra ga, sɩ Thãgbaa iikɛ fɩ-n kʋɛnɩ gɩ. Gɩdonɩ fɛrkɛ dɔnɩ tibil fɩ-n yɩ Thãgba ha fɩ.
43010034	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Sɩ ga khere mɛ̃ anɩ jɔfʋ sɛbɛra gaa ayɩ: “Mɛr Thãgba sɔ ayɩ: Nɛr dʋɔn thãgbasɔaa”?
43010035	Sɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do gɩrɛɛkɛ kherenenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra na puno na kʋɛa', ado anɩ jɔfʋ sɛbɛ n wer thãgbasɔ wɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnanɩ,
43010036	mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ dɩ nɩ so mɛrkɛra Thɩrɛ kɔɔ maanɩ leere kpɩɩ sa thɔ̃ mɩ thɩɩra dɩ nɩ yɩ, mɩ-n kʋɛrɛ Thãgbaa i, gɩdonɩ mɩ kɔɔ so narɛ: Mɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun?
43010037	Ado ma-n cʋʋ ɩ̃ Thɩɩ thɔ̃a', na-n pɛ mɩ haara'.
43010038	Sɩ ado ma cʋʋ gɩrakɛ sɩ dɩ na-n pɛ mɩ haarrakɛ kpɩɩa', nɩ pɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n cʋʋnɩ haar, dɩ mɛ̃ na puno na jɩɩ jɩ dɩ Thɩrɛ har ɩ̃ bɩnɔ dɩ ɩ̃ ha Thɩrɛɛ bɩnɔ.
43010039	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ hʋɛ wo wɩ fʋʋ, sɩ dɩ for awɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
43010040	Jeju bire jal wo Jʋrdɛ̃ mɩɩr iiro, a too kãkɛ Jã n kɔɔ kpɛɛnɩ tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔ cacara.
43010041	Le tɩbɩla bərəəm n pʋɔraa dɩ wa-n so aa: Jã na kɔɔ cʋʋ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ bɩɛla', sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ kuunnaakɛ sobɔr gɩ do.
43010042	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ pɛrɛ Jeju haar dapaalera.
43011001	Kũu bɩɛl gɩ dɩ ga-n khʋʋ. Ɔɔ i n dʋɔn Lajaar; Betanɩ a the Marɩ na ɔɔ õkhɛr Martɩɩ dɩra.
43011002	Marɩɩkɛra dʋɔn ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ thirəni Kɔ̃tɩn latɩkolo, agɩpɩ dɩ pɩɩnʋʋ nɛɛ na ɔɔ yʋsũ. Ɔɔ õkuun ha Lajaarɩkɛra gɩ-n khonɩ.
43011003	Dɩ Lajaarɩ õkhɛrsɔ thɔ̃ a so Jejura ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ʋrɛɛkɛra fɩ nanɩ gɩ-n khʋʋrɛ.
43011004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju nɩɛnɩ ga thɩmɩɩle pɩ a sor: Khoole na do kho kʋnana', sɩ Thãgbaa i ga dʋbɩ, gɩ cʋʋ dakha wɩ dʋbɩ mɛr Thãgbaa Bikuun.
43011005	Sɩ Jeju kɔɔ nar Martɩ, na ɔɔ õkhɛr Marɩ, na awɩ õkuun Lajaar.
43011006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ gɩ-n khor Lajaar, a toore a cʋʋ wire yenyɔ wo kãkɛra a hanɩ.
43011007	Agɩpɩ dɩ so ɔɔ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Sɩ birə jala Jude dɩɩra.
43011008	Dɩ kpãkpãadara sʋʋraa: Dɩɩrdaar, nɛnɛ̃ nɛnɛ̃ Juifisɔ kɔɔ ƴaal wɩ dʋʋrna fɩ bokana sɩ dɩ fa-n bir le woo?
43011009	Dɩ Jeju bule wi: Wi bɩɛl na hana lɩɛr yʋɔr yenyɔaa? Ado tibil na kpaar dɩwɩlʋla, aa-n be nɔa' gɩdonɩ a-n yɩrɛ thɩɩkɛɛ dahɩrɛ.
43011010	Sɩ ado tibil na kpaar dɩtɩnɔ, a-n ber nɔɔ gɩdonɩ dahɩrɛɛ na haaraa ga.
43011011	Ado a mɩɩ wɩ gele pɩ a so warɛ: Asɩ kuun Lajaar daarɛ, sɩ mɩ-n jaal a na jagʋʋ.
43011012	Dɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadara bulee: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado a daarɛ a na ɩɩrɛ.
43011013	Sɩ Lajaarɩ khi Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩ. Sɩ wɛr, wɩ kpɩɛrɛ dɩ dã bʋɔɔkɛ tibil n daarnɩ gɛr Jeju kɔɔ mɩɩ.
43011014	Dɩ Jeju so war dɩphã casɩ: Lajaar khire.
43011015	Sɩ anɩdara daʋ fʋ mɩ gɩrɛraakɛ ma kɔɔ hanɩla', gɩdonɩ ga cʋʋ nɛr dɩ na pɛr haar. Gɛr gɩ sɩ jala ɔɔ pa.
43011016	Dɩ Tomasɩɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Didim so wɩ̃ kpãkpãadarara ayɩ: Nɩ ɩna sɩ jal sɩ khiir kha dakha na Jeju.
43011017	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju n danɩ, a yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ do wɩ 'lire dʋrɛ Lajaar dɩ cɔ we yenã kaʋ.
43011018	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Betanɩ wɔrɔnanɩ Jerujalɛm dɩɩ thɔɔ kilə yẽthersɔ,
43011019	Juifi jɔjʋɔsɔ kɔɔ pɔr Martɩ na Marɩɩ pa wɩ cʋʋ wɩ wɩ faa haar awɩ õkuunidara.
43011020	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Martɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ Jeju har hʋɛra, a ɩɩrɛ da-n caanʋʋ sɩ Marɩ wer toore cʋɔrɔ.
43011021	Dɩ Martɩ so Jejura ayɩ: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado kɛ fɩ kɔɔ ha ɩ̃ õkuun na kɔɔ khə'.
43011022	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛrakɛ mɩ jɩrɛ dɩ thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ fa bɩɛlnɩ Thãgbara, Thãgba na ha fɛr.
43011023	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Afɩ õkuun na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera.
43011024	Dɩ Martɩ birsee: Mɩ jɩrɛ wer dɩ a na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera pɩpɩɩ wirera.
43011025	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Mɛr dʋɔn khi ɩɩrɛ na yire. Ʋrɛɛkɛ n pɛ mɩnɩ haar, ado a khirerakɛ sɩ a na hananɛ yire.
43011026	Dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ hananɩ yire sa pɛ mɩ haar, a na khi yuuə'. Fɩ pɛ gelela haar bɛ?
43011027	Dɩ birsee: Ɔɔ Kɔ̃tɩn, mɩ pɛrɛ haar dɩ fɛr dʋɔn Kirisiti Thãgbaa Bikuun, kɛ ɩnanɩ thɩɩra.
43011028	A Martɩ mɩɩ gelela pɩ, a gbaar jal a we ɔɔ õkhɛr Marɩ a sʋʋraa dɩbara aa: Dɩɩrdaar hakɛ da-n bule fi.
43011029	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Marɩ nɩɛnɩ, a ɩɩrɛ birbir da-n jal Jejura,
43011030	gɩdonɩ Jeju na kɔɔ lõ dɩ bɩnɔ pa', sɩ kãkɛ Martɩ kɔɔ caanʋʋnɩ a ha.
43011031	Dɩ Juifisɔɔkɛ kɔɔ hanɩ kha na Marɩ cɔ bɩnɔ wɩ cʋgʋʋ a faa haar, ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩɩnɩ dɩ ɩɩr birbir da-n the, wɩ kpɩɛrɛ kaara a-n jal a bɩ wo a ɩɩr wa-n kpaaraa.
43011032	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Marɩ danɩ kãkɛ Jeju hanɩ a yɩɩ, a jire ɔɔ ƴɛra sa sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn, ado kɛ fɩ kɔɔ ha ɩ̃ õkuun na kɔɔ khə'.
43011033	Mɔ̃ Jeju yɩɩnɩ da-n khɩɩ nakha Juifisɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ kha, haar kʋɛsʋʋrɛ dɩ ɔɔ kpɩɛr nyanyãa.
43011034	Dɩ Jeju bule: Kana nɩ dʋʋ? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, ɩna hɩnɛ.
43011035	Dɩ Jeju na-n khɩɩ.
43011036	Dɩ Juifisɔ na-n so: Nɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ a thʋnɩ na Lajaar ɓoɓo.
43011037	Sɩ ʋkhasɔ wɛrra na-n so: Ɔrkɛ khɛranɩ yaarʋ yinə, aa kɔɔ puno dakha a cʋʋ kuunikɛ dɩ a na khəə gaa?
43011038	Dɩ haar kʋɛ Jeju wo dɩ gbana da-n jalna kaara. Sɩ gɔ̃gɔ̃ kaar gɩ kɔɔ do dɩ wɩ khaanna bokaar.
43011039	Dɩ Jeju so: Nɩ te bokaar. Dɩ Martɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ khiree õkhɛr sʋʋraa: Kɔ̃tɩn a 'lini phɔɔrɛ pɩrakɛɛ, gɩdonɩ wire yenã a cɔ kaʋ.
43011040	Dɩ Jeju sʋʋraa: Ma kɔɔ so far, ado fɩ pɛr haar fa yɩrɛ Thãgbaa puno hana gaa?
43011041	Dɩ wɩ ti bokaar. Agɩpɩ Jeju gba ƴɩɛ ƴũ sa so: Thɩrɛ, mɩ-n fʋɔr fɛr gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ kɔɔ tuni ɩ̃ bɩɛl.
43011042	Me wer, mɩ jɩrɛrakɛ dɩ fɩ-n ture ɩ̃ bɩɛl wire fɛʋ, sɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ jɩlɛnɩ gɩrɛ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma-n mɩɩ, wɩ pɛr haar dɩ fɛr kɔɔ thɔna mɩ.
43011043	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a mɩɩnɩ gele pɩ, a hulene nɔ kheu: Lajaar, thɛ.
43011044	Dɩ khire the mɔna wɩ kɔɔ paarʋʋnɩ na kẽkẽ gborõbe nƴɛ̃ɛ na nɛɛ, sa paarʋʋ ƴɩɛ na khi dʋ kɩ̃kɩɩn. Dɩ Jeju so war: Nɩ thʋbaa a faa a jal.
43011045	Dɩ Juifi jɔjʋɔɔkɛ kɔɔ pʋɔnnɩ Marɩɩ pa, a wɩ yɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Jeju cʋʋnɩ wɩ pɩɛrɛ haar.
43011046	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn jaal jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔɔ pa, a so war gɩrɛɛkɛ Jeju kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ.
43011047	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ kpar so gʋʋrdara a jɛ sa bule: Anye sa cʋʋ? Gɩdonɩ kũu caakɛ n cʋʋrɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ jɔɔjɔɔ.
43011048	Ado sɩ sɩɩraa da cʋʋ, tɩbɩla fɛʋ na pɩɛrɛ haar, dɩ Rɔmɛ̃sɔ na ɩnɛ na kʋɛ asɩ pa phu na asɩ too.
43011049	Dɩ Kaɩfɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ wɛr bɩɛl, sa do gbõdaar ga yɛraale so warɛ: Na jɩ thɩ̃ɛ kpɩɩraka'.
43011050	Na jɩ dɩɩ do ado tibil bɩɛl khi tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ sora, gɩ baar gɩrɛɛkɛ Juifi caar koo na khiirnəə?
43011051	Sɩ ga do ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ pa gelela a sonɩ tha', sɩ gɩdonɩ ɔr dʋɔn gbõdaar ga yɛɛle, gɛr gɩ dɩ ti Thãgba tukɩrʋ ayɩ: Dɔ Jeju n khi Juifi caarra fɛʋ.
43011052	Sɩ ga do Juifi caar dɩbara dɔ nɔa', sɩ a gbɛbɩ Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔɔkɛ bɩ̃bɩlanɛnɩ paar fɛʋ wɩ do bɩɛl.
43011053	A fʋna ga wiilera wɩ gʋʋrɛ kha mɔ̃ wa kʋnɩ Jeju.
43011054	Gɛr gɩ dɩ Jeju na-n yɩr Juifisɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn gbelẽ gbelẽ bã, sa the le a jal dɩɩraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Efɩraɩm bə̃ khʋra. Dɩ le a too na ɔɔ kpãkpãadara.
43011055	Dɩ Juifisɔɔ Pakɩ n wɔrɔnɛ. Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ the dɩɩra dɩɩra dɩ wa-n jal Jerujalɛm wɩ phʋɔl sɩ fɛtɩ bɔɔ na dã pa'.
43011056	Dɩ le wɩ-n ƴaal Jeju, dɩ wa-n bulena kha bɩɛlbɩɛl Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna aa: Anye nɩ-n kpɩɛr? A na ɩ̃ fɛtɩra gaa?
43011057	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara kɔɔ sor tɩbɩlala, ado tibil jɩrɛ kãkɛ a hanɩ, a sɔ nar ɩnɩ-n fʋʋ.
43012001	Gɩ sɩrɛ we maadõ sɩ Pakɩ n dã, sɩ dɩ Jeju gba jal Betanɩ kãkɛ Lajaarɩkɛ a kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ khirera hanɩ.
43012002	Dɩ le wɩ cʋgʋʋ dɩkor, dɩ Martɩ na-n tɩnɛ wɩ. Lajaar kɔɔ hale dakha na wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hanɩ dɩko kho paar na Jeju.
43012003	Dɩ Marɩ gba latɩkolookɛ n hʋnanɩ daʋ sa khɩɩr the nʋɔ ka litiri kuru, a deer Jejuu nɛra sa pɩɩnʋʋ nɛɛ na ɔɔ yʋsũ, dɩ latɩkolo hʋnɛ tee cʋɔr.
43012004	Sɩ Judasɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Karɩyɔtɩ dɩɩra, kɛ dɔnɩ Jejuu kpãkpãadaar bɩɛlɩkɛ na lirenaanɩ so aa:
43012005	Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ wa kɔɔ dolõ latɩkolookɛ dɩɩ dã wire tãatherɩɩ thɔ̃ lɩmɩ a ha bɔdara ga?
43012006	Sɩ ga do gelela a sonɩ bɔdara a-n kpɩɛrna ga, sɩ gɩdonɩ yu a kɔɔ do a fʋrɔ lokaar da-n yu gɩrɛɛkɛ n lonanɩ.
43012007	Sɩ Jeju so: Sɛ khɛrraakɛ a fʋrɔ latɩkolookɛ a dana wireekɛ wa dʋ mɩnɩ.
43012008	Sɩ ado bɔdara wɛ, wɩ har anɩ pa wire koo, sɩ ado mɛr gɩ ga do wire fɛʋ na hana ma'.
43012009	Dɩ a Juifi jɔjʋɔ nɩɛ dɩ wɩ yɩ Jeju hale Betanɩ, wɩ jaal sɩ ga do Jejuuda dɔ nɔɔ dɩbara ga, sɩ wɩ yɩna dakha Lajaarɩkɛ a kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ khirera.
43012010	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna gʋʋrɛ kha mɔ̃ wa kʋnɩ Lajaar dakha,
43012011	gɩdonɩ Lajaar dɔ nɔɔ dɩ Juifi jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ pɛr Jeju haar sa faa wɩ.
43012012	A dɩɩ wɩl tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ kɔɔ pʋɔnnɩ fɛtɩra, a nɩɛ dɩ wɩ yɩ Jeju na pɔr le Jerujalɛm,
43012013	wɩ gbaar kalã jɛ̃ɛ a thena dɩ wa-n caanʋʋ, sɩ dɩ wa-n hulẽ aa: “Ojana, bɔnanɛ n hana ʋrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa fãgadaar, kɛ n ɩnanɩ gɩrɛ na Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i.”
43012014	Dɩ Jeju yɩ kũkə̃ ɓolʋ a jʋʋn tooro, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ:
43012015	“Na-n do maar n fʋ na' Sɩyɔ̃dara Nɩ hɩnɛ anɩ fãgadaar n pɔr, a jʋʋn kũkə̃ ɓolʋ.”
43012016	Sɩ ɔɔ kpãkpãadarasɔ na kɔɔ jɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔle kɩrʋ pa', sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju kɔɔ birni jʋʋn ɔɔ Thɩɩ dʋɔ pɩ, gɛr wɩ jɩnanɔ dɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ kɔɔ kherenenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra, ɔɔdara gɩ kɔɔ khere, dɩɩ do gɩrɛɛkɛra wɩ cʋʋraanɩ oti gɩ.
43012017	Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ hanɩ kha na Jeju ɔbɔɔkɛ a wenɩ Lajaar kaʋ a ɩɩrʋʋ khirera, wɛr mɩa sobɔ so jɩɩr a pɛ Jejura.
43012018	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ tibil jɔɔle na-n caanʋʋ, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ.
43012019	Dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarasɔ na-n mɩɩ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl awɩ ha: Nɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩ na puno na cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ kpɩɩ bã. Nɩ hɩnɛ, tɩbɩla fɛʋ n kpaaraarɛ.
43012020	Ɩkhaa Gɩrɛkɩsɔɔkɛ hanɩ wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ jalanɩ Jerujalɛm fɛtɩ bɔɔ wɩ fʋɔr Thãgba,
43012021	wɩ pɔr Filipiraakɛ thɛnɩ Galile Bɛcaɩda a bulee: Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩ-n ƴaalɛ sɩ yɩ Jeju.
43012022	Dɩ Filipi jal so Ãdirera, dɩ Ãdire na Filipi gba jal a so Jejura.
43012023	Dɩ Jeju birse wi: Nɩ hɩnɛ, bɔɔkɛ mɛr tibili Bikuun teenanɩ ɩ̃ 'lɛ i dʋbɩrɛ daan.
43012024	Sobɔr mɩ so nar gel, ado ɔljʋ bire na ji thʋnɔ a phu sɩ bire hɩa', a-n toore ɔ bɩɛlla 'lo. Sɩ ado a hɩ a-n ɓaan na sobɔr.
43012025	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n naannɩ ɔɔ yi, ga ka na buurəəre, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n laarɛnɩ ɔɔ yi thɩɩraakɛ, ɔr na ka na 'lɛ gɩ gɩ do yire khorr.
43012026	Ado tibil na do mar thɔma, dɔ a na-n kpa mar, dɩ kãkɛ ma hanɩ le ɩ̃ thɔ̃daar na ha dakha. Ado tibil na do ɩ̃ thɔ̃ Thɩrɛ na cʋʋrɛ.
43012027	Nɛnɛ̃kɛ haar kʋɛ mɛr koo, sɩ anye ma so? Thɩrɛ, taa mɩ bɔ caaraakɛra. Sɩ gelela dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ ɩ̃ a dana bɔ caakɛra.
43012028	Thɩrɛ, dʋba afɩ i. Dɩ le nʋɔ kɔɔ the ƴũ ayɩ: Mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ gɛr dɩ gɩ dʋbɩrɔ, sɩ ma bire na cʋʋ gɩ dɩ ga dʋbɩrɔ wo.
43012029	Dɩ tibil jɔɔkɛ kɔɔ jɩlɛnɩ le, kɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ wɩ sor thãgba tigə. Ɩkhasɔ n yɩ: Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu n mɩanaa.
43012030	Dɩ Jeju so war: Ga do mɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ nɔ caakɛ mɩɩrɔa', sɩ nɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩɩ mɩɩ.
43012031	Nɛnɛ̃kɛ dʋɔn bɔɔkɛ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɩ thɩɩkɛ. Nɛnɛ̃kɛ Thãgba na dʋnanɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩɩkɛɛ fãgadaar na faa.
