44010014	Sɩ Pɩɛr birsee: Kpei Kɔ̃tɩn, gɩdonɩ ma-n kɔɔ kho thɩ̃ sãsɩnanɛ dɩ gɩrɛ biseneni gɩ yuuə'.
44010015	Sɩ a bire nɩ nʋɔra wo balanyɔ dɩɩ sʋʋraa: Gɩrɛ Thãgba yɩnɩ gɩ phure, fa-n hɩɩn gɩ dɩɩ do far thɩ̃ sãsɩnana'.
44010016	Sɩ gɩ bire cʋʋ balãther, sɩ dapaara thɩ̃ɛɛle bire hal jʋʋn thãgbara ƴũ.
44010017	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Pɩɛrɩ kpɩɛr nyanyaanɩ da-n bule ɔɔbara, anye dʋɔn Thãgbaa thɩ̃ yɩrɩlee kɩr ya fɛ, hɩnɛ konaakɛ Kɔrnɛɩ thɔnɩ daan a jɩɩl lõfonʋɔra, dɩ wa-n bule Sɩmɔ̃ɔ cɔ.
44010018	Wɩ wer dɩ wa-n jɩɩ bule ado liir Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pɩɛr n cɔ ger.
44010019	Sɩ mɔ̃ Pɩɛr hanɩ da-n kpɩɛrna Thãgbaa thɩ̃ yɩrɩle, Thu Phuu sʋʋraarɛ: Hɩnɛ, kona yẽther hakɛ dɩ wa-n ƴaal fɩ.
44010020	Ɩrɛ, gbuno nɩ jal kha, sɩ fa-n baalɔa' gɩdonɩ mɛr thɔna wɩ.
44010021	Dɩ mɛ̃ Pɩɛr gbũ a so konanaale: Nɩ hɩnɛ, mɛrra ha ʋ nɩ-n ƴaalnɩ, anye dɔ kɩrʋ nɩ ɩ̃ kɛ?
44010022	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Kɔrnɛɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ dɔnɩ tibil sarʋ da-n ma Thãgba, kɛ Juifi caar fɛʋ n mɩɩnɩ ɔɔda bɔ, ɔr thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ khero gɩrɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara ayɩ, a wɛ fɩ fɩ pɔ ɔɔ cɔ a nɩɛ afɩ thɩmɩɩ.
44010023	Dɩ Pɩɛr kɔɔ kpa wɛr dɩ wɩ cɔ le. A dɩɩ kɔɔ wɩl, a ɩɩrɛ dɩ wɩ jal kha. Sɩ omi ɩkhaakɛ hanɩ Jope kɔɔ thɔɔ wɛr.
44010024	A ʋ̃ dɩ wɩl, wɩ kɔɔ daan Sejare. Sɩ Kɔrnɛɩ wer ɔɔ too na ɔɔ kũu bɩnɔsɔ da-n pɩɛrna wɩ.
44010025	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pɩɛr kɔɔ lonɩ, Kɔrnɛɩ ɩɩrɛ a caanʋʋ a gburõku ɔɔ ƴɛra a fʋɔrʋʋ.
44010026	Sɩ Pɩɛr fʋʋrɛ a khəi dɩ ɩɩr sa sʋʋraa: Ɩrɛ, mee mɛrɛ dakha tibil ha mɩ.
44010027	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Pɩɛr mɩɩnaanɩ sa lõ, a yɩrɛ tɩbɩla jɔɔ dɩ wɩ gbɛbɩ kha le.
44010028	Dɩ so war: Nɩ jɩrɛ gɩ-n sãsɩrɛ Juifira dɩ na too kha na tɩɩ kpalʋ, na dakha dɩ na lõ ɔɔ cɔ, sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ nɩ marɛ ayɩ, ga teena ma-n ƴʋɔn tibil, agɩbo ma-n hɩɩnʋʋ a do mar tɩɩ bisə'.
44010029	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ nɩ thɔnɩ we mɩ dɩ ma hana dɩkha na so bã sa ɩ̃, dɩ nɛnɛ̃ mɩ-n bule ner, anye dɔ kɩrʋ nɩ thɔnɩ we mɩ ɩ̃ ɩna?
44010030	Dɩ Kɔrnɛɩ so: Wire yenã gɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛ nĩ, mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ ɩ̃ cɔ dɩ ma-n bɩɛl Thãgba wi gaara, a na hɩɩn a yɩ tibil bɩɛl dɩ to kẽkẽ bulo dɩ a-n hɩl dɩ jɩɩlna mɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn sa so ayɩ:
44010031	Kɔrnɛɩ, Thãgba nɩɛrɛ afɩ bɩɛl a jɩnana dakha afɩ thɩ̃ 'laa.
44010032	Gɛr gɩ thɔna Jope wɩ we Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pɩɛrɩkɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Sɩmɔ̃ lo kʋdaarɩ cɔ lanyɔ̃ nʋɔra.
44010033	Dɩ dapaara mɩ thʋɔn we fɩ, dɩ mɔ̃ fɩ ɩnɩ thaa, gɩ bɔrɛ. Gɛr gɩ nɛnɛ̃ sɛr ha wɩrɛ fɛʋ kɩɛr Thãgbaa ƴɛra sɩ nɩɛ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Kɔ̃tɩn so farnɩ fɩ mɩa sɩ.
44010034	Le Pɩɛr gba thɩmɩa a mɩɛ wɩ ayɩ: Sobɔr gɩ, mɩ jɩrɛ dɩphã dɩ Thãgba na-n hɩɩn tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa',
44010035	sɩ tibil caarra fɛʋ, ʋrɛɛkɛ n maanɛɛnɩ da-n cʋʋna gɩrɛɛkɛ saranɩ, ɔr n daaraa haar.
44010036	Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsanana a kɔɔ thɔna ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, a mɩɛ wɩ ha ie tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Jeju Kirisitiraakɛra dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn tɩbɩlala fɛʋ.
44010037	Nɩ jɩrɛ gɩrɛ kɔɔ dananɩ Jude dɩɩra fɛʋ, sɩ Galile gɩ kɔɔ tɔ̃tʋɔn ɔbɔɔkɛ Jã kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ yɔ kpɛɛ thɩmɩɩr pɩ.
44010038	Thãgba kɔɔ har Najarɛtɩ Jejura Thu Phuu, a hanaa punone dɩ a-n kpaarɛ paar wo paar da-n cʋʋ bɔɔ, da-n kpɛɛna wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ Satãa nyɔ̃kɔɔ, gɩdonɩ Thãgba kɔɔ hanaanɛ kha.
44010039	Sɛr dɔ sobɔ so jɩdara thɩɛna fɛʋʋkɛ a kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ Juifisɔɔ dɩra na Jerujalɛmna, thɩrʋra wɩ kɔɔ kpaa dɩ khi.
44010040	Sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ ɩɩrʋʋrɛ khirera wire balãther wirera sa cʋgʋʋ dɩ nɩna ɔɔbara,
44010041	sɩ ga do tɩbɩla fɛʋra ga, sɩ sobɔ so jɩdararaakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ maanɩ phiire, kɛ dɔnɩ sɛrkɛ n kɔɔ khɔnɩ kha dɩkor dɩ sa-n yɔna ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ a the khirera.
44010042	Dɩ Jeju kɔɔ pɛ sar sɩ mɩa gɩ tɩbɩla a na kpãkpaanɔ ayɛ, Thãgbaa thɛthɛ kɔɔ phire ni dɩ ɩnɩ do yidara na khee kɩɩldaar.
44010043	Dɩ Thãgbaa bobonasɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ a pɩɛraa ayɩ: Tibil wo tibilikɛ pɩɛnɩ haar, ɔɔ i na dor nɔɔ dɩ na 'lɛrɔ sopugo faarɛ.
44010044	Mɔ̃kɛ Pɩɛr hanɩ mɩɩrɔ, Thu Phuu kɔɔ gbune a lõ wɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ n pɛnɩ thɩmɩɩrɩle nũu.
44010045	Dɩ ha pɛdara fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ khʋ̃ kurdaraakɛ kɔɔ pʋɔnnɩ na Pɩɛr, nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa wɛr gɩrɛraakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ 'laanɩ Thu Phuu wɩrɛraakɛ dʋɔnnɩ ca kpala;
44010046	gɩdonɩ wɩ nɩɛrɛ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩsɔ dɩ wa-n khɩɩna Thãgba.
44010047	Le Pɩɛr bir so: Amɛ na punone na tɔ̃ wɩrɛ 'lɛnɩ Thu Phuu asɩ kha wa-n kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔa?
44010048	Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ so, wɩ kpɛa wɩ nyʋɔnɔ na Jeju Kirisitii i. Dɩ le wɩ bɩɛlɛɛ a tɔɔna nɩ wire gbe wo.
44011001	Thɔ̃thɔna na omɩnaakɛ hanɩ Jude kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ ca kpala dakha kɔɔ 'lɛr Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ.
44011002	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Pɩɛr kɛrnɩ bir Jerujalɛm, ha pɛdaraakɛ dɔnɩ khʋ̃ kurdara kɔɔ ɩɩrnanaanɛ thɩmɩɩr ayɩ,
44011003	a lʋʋn tɩbɩlaakɛ na kuroni khʋ̃aa pa, a khona wɩ dɩkor.
44011004	Dɩ Pɩɛr gba thɩmɩa a mɩɛ wɩ kpa kha kpa kha, mɔ̃kɛ thɩ̃ɛ kɔɔ danɩ ayɩ:
44011005	Jope dɩɩra mɩ kɔɔ ha dɩ ma-n bɩɛl Thãgba a yɩ thɩ̃ yɩr; ɩhɩ̃ɛ gɩ a ho kɩ̃kɩɩn phə̃kərə̃ə dɩ wɩ li li paar yenã, dɩɩ the ƴũ a gbũ dã mɩ.
44011006	Dɩ mɔ̃ mɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ kirkirkir sɩ ma-n kpɩɛr, mɩ yɩrɔrɛ le nɛbi kho thɩ̃ɛ, na nɛkɩɛr sɛ̃bi thɩ̃ɛsɔ thɩɩraakɛ, na hɔ̃ nʋma, na thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ n puuloneni, na 'lominəsɔ.
44011007	Dɩ mɩ nɩɛrɛ nʋɔ dakha kɛ sɔ marnɩ: Pɩɛr, ɩrɛ kʋrɛ a khɔ.
44011008	Sɩ dɩ ɩ̃ birsee: Kpei Kɔ̃tɩn, gɩdonɩ ma kɔɔ kho thɩ̃ sãsɩnanɛ dɩ gɩrɛ biseneni gɩ a lõ mɩ nɔɔ yuuraka'.
44011009	Sɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ bire the ƴũ balanyɔ a so: Gɩrɛ Thãgba yɩnɩ gɩ phure, fa-n hɩɩn gɩ dɩɩ do far thɩ̃ sãsɩnana'.
44011010	Sɩ gɩ kɔɔ bire cʋʋ balãther wo, sɩ agɩpɩ gɩ bire hal koo a lõ thãgbara ƴũ.
44011011	Dɩ dapaara kona yẽtherɩkɛ thɛnɩ Sejare dɩ wɩ thɔ̃ wɩ ɩ̃ pa daan, a jɩɩl cʋɔrɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ hanɩ.
44011012	Dɩ Thu Phuu kɔɔ so marɛ ɩ̃ jalana wɩ sɩ ma-n baalɔa'. Omɩna maadõokɛ kɔɔ thɔɔ mɩ dɩ sɩ kɔɔ jal a lõ Kɔrnɛɩɩ cɔ.
44011013	Dɩ a so sarɛ mɔ̃ a kɔɔ yɩnɩ ɔɔ cɔ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu dɩ jɩɩlaa sa sʋʋraa, a thɔna Jope a wɛ Sɩmɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pɩɛr,
44011014	ɔr na mɩɛnɛɛ thɩmɩasɔɔkɛ na taanɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛ na ɔɔ cɔdara fɛʋ.
44011015	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ manɩ dɩ ma-n mɩɩ, Thu Phuu kɔɔ gbune a lõ war mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ ha sarnɩ dakha fʋ paar mamara.
44011016	Dɩ le mɩ jɩna Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ a sonɩ ayɩ: Nyʋɔnɔ Jã n kɔɔ kpɛɛ tɩbɩla, sɩ ne wer na 'lɛr Thu Phuu kpɛɛrɛ.
44011017	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba ha wɩnɩ khaarda ca bɩɛlla na sɛrɛɛkɛ pɩɛrnɩ Jeju Kirisiti haar, amɛ mɛrkɛ do a na puno na pɩɛr Thãgba?
44011018	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ gele, wɩ pɩrrɛ kɩrkɩrkɩr sɩ wa-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i ayɩ: Dɩ a thale gɩ, Thãgba 'laarɛ ha debire ca kpalala wɩ hanana yire.
44011019	Wɩrɛɛkɛ kpoore kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ dɩ wɩ bɩ̃bɩlã ɔbɔɔkɛ Etɩɛn kɔɔ khini, wɩ kɔɔ jaal a dana Fenɩsɩ, na Sɩpɩr, na Ãtɩyɔsɩ, dɩ wa-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Juifisɔra dɩbara.
44011020	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ wo wɛrraakɛ dɔnɩ Sɩpɩrdara na Sɩrɛndara kɔɔ jaal Ãtɩyɔsɩ a mɩɩna Gɩrɛkɩsɔ a mɩɛ wɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ tutugo bɔda.
44011021	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ fãga kɔɔ ha warɛ, dɩ wɩrɛ kɔɔ pɩɛrnɩ haar a kpa Kɔ̃tɩnna wɩ jɔrɛ ka.
44011022	Dɩ ga tutugoole kɔɔ daan Jerujalɛm we gbɛbɩdara, dɩ wɩ thɔ̃ Barnabasɩ. dɩ pɔ le Ãtɩyɔsɩ.
44011023	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a danɩ le, a yɩrɛ gɩrɛ Thãgba cʋʋnɩ ɔɔ bɔ jɩra dɩ gɩ daaraa, dɩ a kɔɔ mɩɩ wɛr fɛʋ wa-n yɩrana ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal a tɔɔ dakha na ha tɩɩ a ma Kɔ̃tɩnna.
44011024	Gɩdonɩ tibil bʋɔ a do a hinə Thu Phuu na ha pɛrɛ, dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ pɔr Kɔ̃tɩnna.
44011025	Sɩ agɩpɩ Barnabasɩ kɔɔ gbaar jal Tarsɩ a ƴaal Sɔl;
44011026	ɔbɔɔkɛ a yɩɩnɩ, a kpaarɛ dɩ wɩ jal Ãtɩyɔsɩ. Dɩ le wɩ too nakha we gbɛbɩdara dɩ wa-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla bərəəm a cʋʋna yɛ bɩɛl biləni; Ãtɩyɔsɩ dɔ caca bɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ hanɩ kpãkpãadara ire Kirisitii too.
44011027	Ga bɔɔlera Thãgba tukɩr tidara kɔɔ ther Jerujalɛm a jal Ãtɩyɔsɩ.
44011028	Dɩ bɩɛl wɛrraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Agabusi ɩɩrɛ dɩ Thu Phuu kɔɔ cʋgʋʋ dɩ so ayɩ: Kɔmɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na jire thɩɩra fɛʋ. Dɩ gɩ kɔɔ daan bɔɔkɛ Kʋloodɩ kɔɔ dɔnɩ fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ.
44011029	Dɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ gʋʋrɛ kha, sa thɔna thɩ̃ɛ mɔ̃ wɛr bɩɛlbɩɛlɩ puno hanɩ a bulnə omɩnaakɛ hanɩ Jude.
44011030	Dɩ mɛna wɩ kɔɔ gʋʋr sa thɔna Barnabasɩ na Sɔl we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔra.
44012001	Ga bɔɔlera Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar kɔɔ ɩɩrna wɩ̃ we gbɛbɩdarasɔ kpoore,
44012002	a fʋ Jakɩ, Jãa õkuun a kʋ na bajɩna.
44012003	Dɩ mɔ̃ a yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do gɛr n da Juifisɔra, a fʋrɛ Pɩɛr wo a to khaɩra. Buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraa bɔ gɩ kɔɔ do.
44012004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ fʋʋnɩ pɩ, khaɩra a tʋʋ sa pɛr sɔrasɛ yʋɔr maadõ, sɩ yenã yenã wɩ kɔɔ kʋʋr dɩ wa-n bɛrʋʋ kpa kha kpa kha, sa ƴaal a Pakɩ kara wɩ tii wɩ thena tɩbɩlala wɩ kɩɩlnaa.
44012005	Dɩ mɛ̃ Pɩɛr hale khaɩra dɩ wa-n bɛr, sɩ we gbɛbɩdara har dɩ wa-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ Thãgba bɩɛlɛla dɩ wa-n pɩɛraa.
44012006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩ kpɩɛrnɩ ɩna tiirera na thena, ga dɩtɩnɔɔlera Pɩɛr hale da-n daar sɔrasɛ yenyɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn, na jɔrkɔ yenyɔɔkɛ wɩ linəəni, sɩ gardɛsɔ ha lõfonɔɔ dɩ wa-n bɛr khaɩ loo.
44012007	Dɩ hɩnɛ, Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu pɔr dɩ dahɩrɛ carã duu. Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule ber Pɩɛr gɛlʋ a jagʋʋ sa sʋʋraa: Ɩrɛ kɔrɔ. Dɩ jɔrkɔsɔ forʋʋ nyɛɛna a jiir.
44012008	Dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu sʋʋraa: Khɩma afɩ lophɛrɛ, a tɔna afɩ nɛfaa. Dɩ cʋʋ oti. Dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuulera bir sʋʋraa wo: Tɔ afɩ darã sɩ na kpa mar.
44012009	Dɩ Pɩɛr the da-n kpaaraa, sɩ aa jɩɛ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule n cʋʋnɩ thɩ̃ɛ gɩ sobɔra', a ka jɩna thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ ɩnɩ yɩ.
44012010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kpãasɛnɩ caca gardɛra na balanyɔdarara, wɩ daan lõfonʋɔɔkɛ wɩ-n thenanɩ dɩɩra, kɛ wɩ-n khaananɩ the loo, dɩ loole khɛr warɛ dɩbara, dɩ wɩ thɩɩr a gba hʋ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dɩ wa-n jal. Dɩ dapaara Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule faarɛ Pɩɛr.
44012011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pɩɛr jɩnɩ tue a sor: Mɩ jɩrɛ dɩphã waa dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn thɔna ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu dɩ taa mɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ na gɩrɛra fɛʋʋkɛ Juifisɔ n pɛnɩ nũu.
44012012	A kpɩɛrnɩ thale na pɩ, a gbaar jal Marɩɩ cɔ; Jãakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Markɩɩ nɩ gɩ, ka tɩbɩla bərəəm gbɛbɩnɩ kha dɩ wa-n bɩɛl Thãgba.
44012013	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a benɩ phel ko loo, thɔ̃daar khɛ bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Rɔɔdɩ pɔrra a jɩ ntɛ.
44012014	Dɩ a jɩrɛ Pɩɛrɩ wi; dɩ daʋ na-n haa lo khɛrʋa', dɩ ca bir so aa: Pɩɛr hale lõfonɔɔ.
44012015	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Yʋʋ bo fɩ yaa? Sɩ dɩ bo da-n ɩɩrɔ aa, gɩrɛ ɩnɩ sonɩ ɔmɛ̃ gɩ. Dɩ wɩ so: Ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu ga do.
44012016	Sɩrakɛ Pɩɛr har da-n be loo. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ khɛrnɩ loo a yɩɩ nʋɔ kpaa wɛr.
44012017	Sɩ a jɛ wɛr na nyɛ̃ɛ wɩ pɩra, sa mɩɛ wɩ mɔ̃ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ cʋgʋʋnɩ dɩ the khaɩra. Sɩ a sor wo ayɩ, wɩ sɔ Jakɩra na omɩnana thɩ̃ɛɛlera. Sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ the da-n jal dɩkhãa pa.
44012018	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ kpɛɛnɩ, khʋ̃ɛ kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ sɔrasɛɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ aa: Mɔ̃ Pɩɛr do ya fɛ?
44012019	Dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ ƴaalʋʋlɛ ƴaal ƴaal ƴaal sɩ aa kɔɔ yɩa', dɩ a kɩɩlnanɛ gardɛsɔ sa 'laa hʋɛ wɩ kʋrɛ wɩ. A gele pɩ, Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ ther Jude a jal Sejare a too.
44012020	Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ hananɛ sor na Tɩɩrdara na Sɩdɔ̃dara. Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ gʋʋrɛ kha nɔ bɩɛl sa pɔna dɩkha a kurnə kuune na Bɩlasɩtɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaarɩ du hɩɩndaar, sa jal Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ pa a ƴɛgʋʋ ha ɩɩ n hana le gɩdonɩ fãgadaarɩ dɩɩle n haanɛ wɩ.
44012021	Dɩ Ɛrɔɔdɩ kɔɔ dʋrɛ wire sa to ɔɔ fãgadaar kẽkẽ a toona ɔɔ fãga too pa, a mɩɩ thɩmɩɩr tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra.
44012022	Dɩ tɩbɩla thʋ̃ hulẽ aa, ga do tibil n mɩa bã sɩ Thãgba a ho mɛ̃.
44012023	Dɩ le dapaara Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɩ, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa i a fi tee. Dɩ dokora ɩɩrnaanɛ dɩ khi.
44012024	Sɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ so kpaarɛ a ƴɛr dɩ a-n pɛr.
44012025	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Barnabasɩ na Sɔl kɔɔ donɩ awɩ thɔ̃ pɩ, wɩ kɔɔ ther Jerujalɛm sɩ wɩ kɔɔ kpar Jãakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Markɩ a fʋrɔ kɔna.
44013001	Thãgba tukɩr tidara na dɩɩrdara kɔɔ har we gbɛbɩdararaakɛ hanɩ Ãtɩyɔsɩ; Barnabasɩ na Sɩmɛ̃ʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ tɩɩ biru, na Lusiyusiikɛ thɛnɩ Sɩrɛn, na Manahɛnɩkɛ wɩ haananɩ kha Ɛrɔɔdɩ fãgadaar buu, na Sɔl.
44013002	Mɔ̃kɛ wɩ lini nʋɔ dɩ wa-n fʋɔrna Kɔ̃tɩn, Thu Phuu sor: Nɩ lea mar Barnabasɩ na Sɔl kpɩɩ thɔmanaakɛ mɩ we warnɩ.
44013003	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ lini nʋɔ sa bɩɛl Thãgba pɩ, wɩ dɛ̃ɛ warɛ nyɛ̃ɛ sa sɩ war dɩ wɩ jal.
44013004	Dɩ mɔ̃ Thu Phuu thɔnɩ Barnabasɩ na Sɔl, mɛ̃ wɩ jal a dã Seləsɩ, dɩ le wɩ gba bato a jal Sɩpɩr.
44013005	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ danɩ Salamɩn, wɩ kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ; sɩ Jã wɩ kɔɔ hana kha da-n bul wi.
44013006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpaarnɩ yɔ dɩɩle fɛʋ a pɩ sa dã Pafɔsɩ, le wɩ kɔɔ caana Juifi dɔdɔɔdaar bɩɛlɩkɛ n sõsonenɩ dɩ yɩ bobon ha nɩ. Ɔɔ i n dʋɔn Barjeju;
44013007	a kɔɔ har kha na Sɛrjiyusi Polusiikɛ dɔnɩ gobanɛr, kɛ jɩɛnnɩ thɩ̃ɛ ka. Gobanɛrɩle kɔɔ wer Barnabasɩ na Sɔl, gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ ƴaalɛ ka a nɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ.
44013008	Sɩ Elɩmasɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ dɔdɔɔdaar, thale dɔ ɔɔ i na gɩrɛkɩ thɩmɩɩr, a-n bãbarã wɛr da-n ƴaal a pɩɛr gobanɛrɩle a na-n pɛ haara'.
44013009	Sɩ Sɔlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ dakha Pol hinəne Thu Phuu da-n hɩɩn Elɩmasɩ kirkirkir sa sʋʋraa ayɩ:
44013010	Fɛrɛɛkɛ gõgolone na fɩɩlɛ n theronɩ, fɛr Satãa bi, fɛr fɩl sar lãlaardaar, fa thʋ̃ na sɩrɔ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋ sarra fɩ-n golonaa?
44013011	Nɛnɛ̃ fa yɩ gaa, Kɔ̃tɩn na ga farɛ ɔɔ nyɔ̃bi dɩ fa yaar, fa yɩ wirə' phaphapha gɩ dana bɔɔ gbe. Dɩ dapaara dɩɩ haaraa gbibi dɩ dabirə thiirəə da-n bəər, dɩ le a ƴaal tɩbɩla dɩ wa-n halʋʋ.
44013012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ gobanɛr yɩnɩ gele dananɩ, a pɛrɛ haar sɩ nʋɔ kɔɔ kpagʋʋrɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ dɩɩra.
44013013	Pol kɔɔ ther Pafɔsɩ na ɔɔ kpakpaarsɔ a lõ bato a jal Pãfɩlɩ Pɛɛrjɩ dɩɩra. Sɩ Jã kɔɔ faa wɛr sa kɛr bir Jerujalɛm.
44013014	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ ther Pɛɛrjɩ wo a gba hʋɛ a jal Pisidi Ãtɩyɔsɩ. Dɩ hɩɩr wire wɩ kɔɔ lʋʋn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra a too.
44013015	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ sonɩ jɔfʋ na Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ sɛbɛ a pɩ, wɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩna Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra thʋɔn bule wi aa: Omɩna, ado nɩ hananɛ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ na hananɩ tɩbɩla ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal, nɩ mɩa wɩ.
44013016	Le Pol ɩɩr a jɛ tibɩla na nyɛ̃ɛ wɩ pɩra sa so war: Nɛr Ɩjɩrayɛldara, na nɛrkɛ n maannɩ Thãgba, nɩ pɛ nũu.
44013017	Ɩjɩrayɛl Thãgba kɔɔ phire asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, dɩ a cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wɩ ler ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ donɩ kpakpala Ejipiti dʋɔ, agɩpɩ dɩ pɛr ɔɔ fãga nyɛ̃ a ti wi le.
44013018	Dɩ a kɔɔ fʋ warɛ haar a cʋʋna yɛna kpalanyɔ le bəənnə,
44013019	dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ bũburoni caar makonyɔ Kanãa dɩɩra, a gbaar awɩ dɩ a ha ɔɔ too.
44013020	Gɩ pʋɔrɛ a thɔɔ yɛna taanã na kpalanyɔ yʋɔr. A gele pɩ, a kɔɔ ha wɛr so kɩɩldara dɩɩ dana Samʋɛl Thãgbaa bobonɩ bɔɔ.
44013021	Dɩ agɩpɩ wɛr kɔɔ bɩɛlnɛ fãgadaar. Dɩ Thãgba ha wɛr Sayʋl, Kɩsɩɩ bikuun, kɛ dɔnɩ Bɛ̃jamɛ̃ɛ ca dɩ do war fãgadaar a cʋʋna yɛna kpalanyɔ.
44013022	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ bʋʋnɩ faa, a kɔɔ gbaar Davɩdɩ a ha wɩ dɩ do fãgadaar. Ɔr a mɩɩrɔ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ ayɩ: “Mɩ yɩrɛ Davɩdɩ Ɩjaɩɩ bikuun dɩphã, tibil gɩ a ha mɔ̃ ɩ̃ bɩ̃ pɛrnɩ haar, ɔr na cʋɛ ɩ̃ tuur fɛʋ.”
44013023	Dɩ Davɩdɩɩ məlla Thãgba kɔɔ cʋʋ Taadaarɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju dɩ the, dɩ ha Ɩjɩrayɛldara mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ ʋlfɛ hanɩ.
44013024	Ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ ɩnɩ pa', Jã n kɔɔ mɩa Ɩjɩrayɛldarara fɛʋ aa: Nɩ deba haar sa 'lɛ yɔ kpɛɛrɛ.
44013025	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Jãa thɔ̃ n wɔrɔnɩ pɩr, gɛr a kɔɔ sor ayɩ: Ma do tibil ʋrɛ nɩ-n pɛrnɩ haar gɩrɛ mɩ dora', sɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, tibil bɩɛl hale a na kpa mar, kɛ ma teenanɩnakɛ ɩ̃ fʋʋrʋʋ nɛfaa ga.
44013026	Omɩna, nɛrkɛ dɔnɩ Abɩrahamɩ məl na wɩrɛ hanɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn kɛ n maannɩ Thãgba, sɛrra wɩ thɔna taa thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ.
44013027	Gɩdonɩ Jerujalɛmdara na awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ na kɔɔ jɩ Jeju, dɩ Thãgbaa bobonaa thɩmɩɩkɛ wɩ-n sonɩ wire fɛʋ hɩɩr wire ga, dɩ mɔ̃ wɩ kɔɔ heenuuni sor, wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ sonɩ ga har.
44013028	Sɩ gɩdonɩ wa yɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ dɩɩ teena wɩ kʋa', sɩrakɛ wɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ Pɩlatɩ a kʋɔ.
44013029	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ ha mɔ̃ gɩ khereraanɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra, agɩpɩ wɩ gbuune kʋkʋ thɩrʋra a dʋ.
44013030	Sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ ɩɩrʋʋrɛ khirera.
44013031	Dɩ wire jɔɔjɔɔ a-n kɔɔ nɩnanɛ ɔɔbara wɩrɛɛkɛ a-n kɔɔ thenanɩ kha Galile da-n jal Jerujalɛm, kɛ dɔnɩnakɛ gɩrɛ ɔɔ sobɔ so jɩdara tɩbɩlala.
44013032	Dɩ sɛrɛ, sɩ-n mɩɩ narɛ ga tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩkɛ dɩ sɩ yɩ, gɩrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ,
44013033	a kɔɔ cʋʋ gɛr dɩɩ da otirə; dɩ ha sɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ awɩ bɩsãsɔ mɔ̃ a kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ Jeju khirera mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Khɩkhɩɩ nɩɛsɔ yenyɔra ayɩ: “Fɛr dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuun, mɛr Thãgba kɔna fɩ nĩ gɩrɛ.”
44013034	Dɩ a kɔɔ ɩɩrʋʋrɛ khirera dɩ mɛ̃ a na bir kʋɛrɛra ga, gɩdonɩ gɛrra a kɔɔ so ayɩ: “Mɛr Thãgba na ha nɛr thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ phonɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ Davɩdɩɩdaakɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ waa gel.”
44013035	Dɩ gɛr gɩ gɩ bire so Thãgbaa sɛbɛra dɩkhãa pa wo ayɩ: “Fa tu dɩ afɩ Tɩɩ phu na yɩ kʋɛra'.”
44013036	Dɩ Davɩdɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ Thãgbaa tuur ɔɔ bɔraalera pɩ, a kɔɔ khire dɩ wɩ dʋʋ ɔɔ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ kara dɩ yɩ kʋɛrɛ.
44013037	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ wer Thãgba kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ khirera, aa kɔɔ yɩ kʋɛra'.
44013038	Gɛr gɩ, nɛr omɩna, nɩ jɩɛ jɩ bɔɔbɔɔ dɩ sopugo faarɛɛkɛ wɩ-n mɩɩ narnɩ ɔɔ pa gɩ the;
44013039	sorɩkɛ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ na kɔɔ punoni na hɛl nara', ʋrɛɛkɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar ɔrra, sorra na hɛlaalɛ.
44013040	Gɛr gɩ na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ dɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa bobona kɔɔ sonɩ na dã na'. Gɩdonɩ gɩ sor:
44013041	“Nɩ hɩnɛ, nɛr tɩɩ beesidara, nɩ dɔ nʋɔ n kpaa nɩ, dɩ dakha nɩ bũburone. Gɩdonɩ mɛr Thãgba na cʋʋrɛ thɔ̃ bɩɛl anɩ bɔra, thɔma gɩ ado wa mɩɩ nar na pɛr haara'.”
44013042	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol na Barnabasɩ n thenɩ, wɩ bire ƴaal wɩ wɩ birə mɩa ga thɩmɩɩle hɩɩr wireekɛ n kpaanɛnɩ.
44013043	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ thenɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ, Juifisɔ bərəəm na kpakpalaakɛ fenɩ ho Juifisɔ, kɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Thãgba n kpar Polla na Barnabasɩra dɩ wa-n khʋɛ kha, dɩ wɩ kɔɔ yɩrna wɛr ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal dɩ wa mar yʋʋ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩra.
44013044	Hɩɩr wireekɛ n kpaanɛnɩ, fɩɩʋ sɛ sɩɩ do tɩbɩla dɩɩraale koo gbɛbɩrɛra kha a pɛ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ nũu.
44013045	Sɩ mɔ̃ Juifisɔ yɩnɩ tibil jɔɔle, gbugi fʋlɛ wɛr dɩ wa-n bana thɩ̃ banaa gɩrɛraakɛ Pol sonɩ dɩ wa-n kʋɛnaa ire.
44013046	Dɩ le Pol na Barnabasɩ so war na 'lar ayɩ: Nɛr Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ kɔɔ teena gɩ mɩa ɓo, sɩ gɩdonɩ nɩ bor sa hɩɩn anɩbara dɩɩ do yire khorr na teena na', gɛr gɩ nɩ hɩnɛ, ca kpalaa pa sɩ-n jal gɩrɛ.
44013047	Gɩdonɩ mɛ̃ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ 'laa sar jɔfʋ ayɩ: “Mɩ thɩɩn fɛr fɩ do dahɩrɛ tibil caar fɛʋra, dɩ fa gba taarɛ na jalna gɩ dana ka thɩɩ khuni.”
44013048	Dɩ ca kpala n kãkarɛ mɔ̃ wɩ nɩɛnɩ gele. Dɩ wɩ-n kpãgarɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ so, dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba phiirni dɩ wa 'lɛ yire khorr kɔɔ pɩɛr haar.
44013049	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ so kɔɔ kpaarɛ dɩɩraale koo.
44013050	Khɛraakɛ jɩɛnnɩ too, kɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Thãgba dakha, Juifisɔ kɔɔ cʋr wɛr pɛr na kɔ̃tɩna dɩɩra dɩ wɩ ɩɩrna kpoore Polla na Barnabasɩra, a wee wɩ le ɩwɩ dɩra a faa.
44013051	Dɩ wɛr dakha kɔɔ kpɛɛrɛ thɩlãkobeekɛ ma wɩnɩ nɛɛ a faa war, sa gba jal Ɩkɔn.
44013052	Sɩ ado kpãkpãadara wer gɩ, daʋ na Thu Phuu kɔɔ he war.
44014001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol na Barnabasɩ kɔɔ danɩ Ɩkɔn, wɩ kɔɔ lʋʋn le Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra mɔna wɩ-n kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ, a thʋ̃ mɩɩ thɩmɩɩr, dɩ Juifisɔ bərəəm na Gɩrɛkɩsɔ pɛr haar.
44014002	Sɩ Juifisɔɔkɛ na-n tuonni dɩ wa pɛr haara', wɩ ɩɩrɛ cʋr ca kpala a pɛr wɩ cʋɛ omɩna puure.
44014003	Sɩ Pol na Barnabasɩ kɔɔ toore Ɩkɔn a pʋɔr dɩ wa-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ na 'lar gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnna wɩ ƴɛl; dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn ture ɔɔ bɔ jɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ wɩ-n mɩɩnɩ dɩ sobɔr gɩ do, a ha wɛr dakha punone dɩ wa-n cʋʋna nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔ.
44014004	Sɩ dɩdara kɔɔ tɩnɛnɛ dɩ wɛ hana Juifisɔ, sɩ wɛ hana thɔ̃thɔna.
44014005	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ ca kpala, na Juifisɔ, na awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ gʋʋrnɩ kha sa ɩɩrna kpoore Polla na Barnabasɩra dɩ wa-n dʋʋrna wɩ bokana,
44014006	wɩ fuure jal Likaʋnɩ dɩɩsɔraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Lisitiri na Dɛɛrbɩ na yɛ̃ dɩsɔraakɛ khonanɩ le.
44014007	Dɩ le wɩ too dɩ wa-n mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ.
44014008	Sɩ kũu bɩɛl kɔɔ hale Lisitiri dɩ ɔɔ nɛ khi; wɩ kʋɔnɛ na gbãgbarɛ dɩ aa kɔɔ sarakɛ thɩɩ a jal a yɩ ga.
44014009	Dɩ a-n kɔɔ pɛ nũu ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol n kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ, sɩ Pol n hɩɩnʋʋnɛ kirkirkir a yɩɛ a jɩ dɩɩ do a hananɛ ha pɛrɛɛkɛ na kpɛɛnɛɛnɩ,
44014010	a so nɔ khɩɩr ayɩ: Ɩrɛ jɩlɛ kɩbɩ na nɛɛ; dɩ dapaara dɩ pal ɩɩr a ma da-n sa.
44014011	Mɔ̃ tibil jɔ yɩnɩ gɩrɛ Pol cʋʋnɩ, wɩ-n hulene na Likaʋnɩ thɩmɩɩr ayɩ: Thãgbasɔ gbuno kɛ asɩ pa a ho tɩbɩla.
44014012	Dɩ wɩ-n wer Barnabasɩ Jəsi, sɩ Pol na-n do Ɛrmɛsɩ gɩdonɩ ɔr n mɩa thɩmɩa.
44014013	Dɩ lõfonʋɔra Jəsii fʋɔr cɔ kɔɔ ha; dɩ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ Jəsii gbõdaar kɔɔ kpar nakenaakɛ wɩ tonɩ sʋkparasɔɔkɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ thɩr phɩ̃ɩ a pɔna lõfonʋɔra, dɩ a ƴaalɛ ɔr, na tibil jɔɔle n je Polsɔra bonɩɛ.
44014014	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ thɔ̃thɔnaale Barnabasɩ na Pol kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ gele, wɩ ɓəəre awɩ kẽkẽsɔ sa ca birbir lõ tibil jɔraalee thɩ̃thɩɩn a hulẽ:
44014015	Kona, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n cʋʋ gɩrɛ? Sɛrɛ dakha tɩbɩlala sɩ do mɔ̃ nɩ hanɩ, dɩ sa-n mɩɩ nar tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩr dɩ sɩ yɩ, gɩ teenanɛ dɩ na faa mɔlɔ thɩlasɔɔkɛ sɩ nɩ kɛr nɩ pɛ Thãgba haar, ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ yidaar, kɛ kɔɔ tenɩ ƴũ, na thɩɩ, na lanyʋɔn, na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ha garnɩ bɩnɔ.
44014016	Dɩ bɔɔkɛ kɔɔ kanɩ, a kɔɔ sɩrɛ tibil caarra fɛʋ wa-n jalana awɩ hʋ,
44014017	sɩrakɛ aa kɔɔ faarakɛ nɩnanɛɛkɛ a-n nɩnanɩ ntɛ a dona'; a-n nɩna nɛr ɔɔ bɔ cʋʋ mɔ̃ a-n 'laa narnɩ nyʋɔn na yɛ bʋɔ, da-n hana nɩ dakha dɩkɔ jɔɔjɔɔ na daʋ anɩ hara.
44014018	Sɩrakɛ thɔ̃thɔnaale mɩɩ wɩnɩ thale, sɩ ga khe war kpãkpalã sɩ dɩ wɩ mar a pɩɛr tibil jɔɔle dɩ wa jɩ war bonɩaa ga.
44014019	Agɩpɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ ther Ãtɩyɔsɩ na Ɩkɔn a pɔ a fɩɩl tibil jɔ pɛr, dɩ wɩ dʋʋr Pol na bokana sa halʋʋ thena dɩ khuirə, a ka jɩna a khire.
44014020	Dɩ mɔ̃ kpãkpãadara kpanɩ jɛ a diirəə, a pallɛ ɩɩr a bir lõ le dɩɩra. A dɩɩ wɩl Pol gbaar jal Dɛɛrbɩ na Barnabasɩ.
44014021	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ mɩɩnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ dɩɩraale a cʋʋna tɩbɩla jɔɔ dɩ wɩ do kpãkpãadara, wɩ kɛrrɛ bir Lisitiri, na Ɩkɔn, na Ãtɩyɔsɩ;
44014022	dɩ wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ kpãkpãadara dɩ wɩ tɩ, dɩ wɩ yɩrna wɛr wɩ yɩra tɔɔ ha pɛrɛra, wɩ so warɛ dakha ayɩ, dɔ sɩ yɩ bɔ gaarɛ jɔɔ sɩ sɩ lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩra.
44014023	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ phiire we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ a pɛ we gbɛbɩdarara paar fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl; ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ lini nʋɔ a bɩɛlna Thãgba a pɛ war, wɩ faa wɛr Kɔ̃tɩnnaakɛ wɩ kɔɔ pɛrnɩ haarɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
44014024	Agɩpɩ wɩ jaal the Pisidi sa gba pɔ Pãfɩlɩ.
44014025	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ mɩɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Pɛɛrjɩ pɩ, wɩ gbaar jal Atalɩ.
44014026	Le wɩ kɔɔ gba bato a jal Ãtɩyɔsɩ, ka wɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba a bɔna wɩ thɔmanaakɛ wɩ pɩnɩ gele.
44014027	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ danɩ, wɩ wer we gbɛbɩdara a der pa bɩɛl a mɩɛ wɩ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba gba wɩnɩ a cʋʋna, na mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ khɛrnɩ hʋɛ ca kpalala dɩ wa pɛr haar.
44014028	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ toore na kpãkpãadara a pʋɔr.
44015001	Ɩkhaa tibilsɔ kɔɔ ther Jude a pɔ a dɩɩr omɩna ayɩ: Ado na-n kur khʋ̃ʋ mɔ̃kɛ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ n sona', na puno na 'lɛ taara'.
44015002	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Pol na Barnabasɩ na-n tunə', wɩ ɩɩrnanɛ kha thɩ̃ banaa; dɩ omɩna kɔɔ gʋʋrɛ kha sa yɩ, Pol na Barnabasɩ na awɩ tibil ɩkhasɔ n jala Jerujalɛm thɔ̃thɔnana na we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ pa thɩ̃ banaanaalera.
44015003	Dɩ we gbɛbɩdara kɔɔ thɔɔ wɛr a pɛ hʋɛra, dɩ wɩ kpaarɛ Fenɩsɩ na Samarɩ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ mɔ̃kɛ ca kpala kɛrnɩ dɩ wa-n kpa Thãgbara, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ dar omɩnasɔra fɛʋ ka.
44015004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ danɩ Jerujalɛm we gbɛbɩdara, na thɔ̃thɔna, na we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ tee wer, dɩ wɩ kɔɔ mɩɛ wɛr thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ gba wɩnɩ a cʋʋna.
44015005	Sɩ wɛ hale wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara awɩ ƴɛra kpɩɩ, kɛ kɔɔ pɩɛrnɩ haar, wɛr ɩrɛ a so ayɩ, dɔ wa-n kur ca kpala khʋ̃ʋ, sɩ wɩ so war wa-n hɩɩn Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ.
44015006	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔna na we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kpar gbɛbɩrɩ kha wɩ gʋʋr thɩmɩɩrɩle.
44015007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ bananɩ kha jɔɔ pɩ, Pɩɛr ɩɩrɛ a so war: Omɩna, nɩ jɩrɛ gɩ maanɛ gɩrɛ ka Thãgba phiir mini anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn dɩ ma-n mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ ca kpalala wɩ pɛr haar;
44015008	dɩ Thãgbaakɛ n jɛnɩ tɩbɩlaa ha, a nɩna wɛr mɔ̃ a tee wɩnɩ a hana wɩ Thu Phuu mɔna a ha sɩnɩ;
44015009	aa hana dɩɩdɩɩ hɩɩnɛ sɛrɛ na wɛrra ga, gɩdonɩ a cʋʋrɛ awɩ ha dɩɩ phu dɩɩ the ha pɛrɛra.
44015010	Dɩ nɛnɛ̃ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n fifilə Thãgba nɩ hɩɩn a ƴaal nɩ heen kpãkpãadara heendaakɛ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, dɩ sɛr gɩ, na kɔɔ punoni a heena?
44015011	Sɩ Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩnɩ bɔ jɩra sɩ pɛr haar a 'lɛ taarɛ mɔ̃ wɩ 'lɛnɩ taarɛ.
44015012	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle pɩrrɛ kɩrkɩrkɩr sɩ wa-n pɛ Pol na Barnabasɩ nũu, kɛ n mɩa wɩnɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ Thãgba gba wɩnɩ a cʋʋna ca kpalaa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
44015013	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ mɩɩnɩ pɩ, Jakɩ gbaar thɩmɩɩr a so ayɩ: Omɩna, nɩ pɛ ɩ̃da nũu.
44015014	Sɩmɔ̃ so sarɛ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ hɩɩnnɩ ca kpala caca bɔɔlera, sa phiir tɩbɩla awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn kɛ na-n wɛnɩ ɔɔ i.
44015015	Dɩ Thãgbaa bobonaa thɩmɩɩ fʋrɛ kha na gelela, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ ayɩ:
44015016	“A gele pɩ, mɛr Thãgba na bire na ɩ̃; a na bir na dʋ Davɩdɩɩ waakɛ kɔɔ jenɩ. Ma bire na dʋ ɔɔ dakʋɛ, ma bire na gbɛbɩ gɩ wo.
44015017	Dɩ mɛ̃ tɩbɩlaakɛ sɛnɩ na ƴaal mɛr Kɔ̃tɩn; mɛna gɩ na tibil caar fɛʋʋkɛ n fʋɔrɛ mɩnɩ.
44015018	Mɛr Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ dɩɩ do gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dajɩnanɛ khorr sɔ.”
44015019	Gɛr gɩ, ka mer yɩna gɩnɩ, gɩ bɔrɛ dɩ sa-n gba nɩwɛ a heen wɩrɛ thɛnɩ ca kpalaa pa a kɛr a pɛ Thãgba haara'.
44015020	Sɩ sɩ kherene sɛbɛ a sɔ war, wɩ bɔ thɩl thĩ khor, na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ, wa-n kho dakha nʋmɩkɛ khenɩ sɩ tɔmɩn na thaa ga, wa-n kho dakha tɔmɩna'.
44015021	Gɩdonɩ gɩ maanɛ kɛkɛkɛ tɩbɩla kɔɔ hanɩle dɩɩ dɩɩra dɩ wa-n so Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ. Hɩɩr wire fɛʋ wɩ-n gɩ sɛbɛra Juifiisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra.
44015022	Dɩ le thɔ̃thɔnasɔ, na we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, na we gbɛbɩdara fɛʋ dakha yɩɛrɛ aa, gɩ bɔrɛ ɩnɩ-n phiir tɩbɩla ɩnɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn ɩnɩ-n thɔ̃ wɩ Ãtɩyɔsɩ nakha Pol, na Barnabasɩ, na Juudiikɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Barsabasɩ, nakha Sɩlasɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ hananɩ i bʋɔ omɩnaa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
44015023	Dɩ wɩ kherere sɛbɛ a ha wɩ ayɩ: Sɛr omɩnaakɛ dɔnɩ thɔ̃thɔna, na we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, kherene sɛbɛɛkɛ a thɔna omɩnanaakɛ thɛnɩ ca kpalaa pa kɛ hanɩ Ãtɩyɔsɩ, na Siri, na Silisi ayɩ: Nɩ gba fʋɔrɛ.
44015024	Mɔ̃ sɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ thɛnɩ asɩ pa, kɛ sa kɔɔ soronɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛllaka', awɩ thɩmɩɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ nɛr kpɩɛrɛ dɩɩ nyanyãa dɩ haar fi ni;
44015025	dɩ gɛr gɩ sɩ kɔɔ gʋʋr kha, a do nɔ bɩɛl, a yɩɛ dɩɩ bɔr dɩ sɩ kɔɔ phiir tɩbɩlaakɛ, a thɔ̃ wɩ anɩ pa na Barnabasɩ na Polɩkɛ sɩ-n nanɩ,
44015026	kɛ dɔnɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ faanɩ awɩ yi dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i dɔ nɔɔ.
44015027	Sɩ thʋɔn dakha Juudi na Sɩlasɩ, wa mɩɩ nɛr ɔmɛna na awɩ nɔ.
44015028	Gɩdonɩ Thu Phuu yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ bɔr, dɩ sɛrɛ dakha mɛ̃ sɩ yɩɛ, dɩ sa-n pɛ nar heendaa saagado thɩ̃ doo teere kha gaaga, dɩ gɩrɛ teanɩ kha dʋɔn:
44015029	Nɩ bɔ bonɩ ji nʋʋn, na tɔmɩn, na nʋmɩkɛ khenɩ sɩ tɔmɩn na tha', na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ, thɩ̃ɛ gɩɩkɛ na n jɩɩnɩ dʋrɔ bʋrɛ, na-n cʋa'. Nɩ tɔɔ bɔɔ.
44015030	Sɩ wɛr, ɔbɔɔkɛ we gbɛbɩdara kɔɔ fʋɔr wɩnɩ pɩ, gɛr wɩ jaal Ãtɩyɔsɩ a kpa tibil jɔ a jɛ sa ha wɩ sɛbɛɛle.
44015031	Ɔbɔɔkɛ omɩnaale hɩɩnnɩ sɛbɛɛle pɩ, daʋ fʋ wɛr ha faarɛraale wɩ 'lɛnɩ.
44015032	Dɩ Juudi na Sɩlasɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgba tukɩr tidara, wɛr kɔɔ mɩa omɩnaale thɩmɩa jɔɔ dɩɩ ha wɩ ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal a cʋʋna wɩ dɩ wɩ tɩ dakha.
44015033	A gɩ pʋɔr gbe, omɩnaale kɔɔ sɩ warɛ na ha ɩɩ dɩ wɩ bir kɔ̃ wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ thɔna wɩnɩɩ pa.
44015034	[Sɩ Sɩlasɩ or, a yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ bɔr dɩ too.]
44015035	Pol na Barnabasɩ toore Ãtɩyɔsɩ dɩ wa-n dɩɩr tɩbɩla, dɩ wa-n mɩɩna Kɔ̃tɩnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ na tibil jɔ.
44015036	Ɔbɔɔkɛ ga pʋɔrnɩ gbe, gɛr Pol sor Barnabasɩra ayɩ: Sɩ kɛra birə a yɛ omɩna dɩɩsɔ fɛʋraakɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ so, a hɩnɛ a jɛ mɔ̃ wɩ hanɩ.
44015037	Dɩ Barnabasɩ or ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n kpa Jãakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Markɩ a fɔrɔ,
44015038	sɩ Pol yɩɛrɛ dɩ ga bɔr dɩ ɩna kpa ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ faa nɩnɩ Pãfɩlɩ, kɛ na kɔɔ thɔɔ nɩnɩ thɔmana ga, a jalana ga.
44015039	Dɩ thɩ̃ banaale kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a khɩɩr ka, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ lee kha, dɩ Barnabasɩ kpa Markɩ dɩ wɩ ha kha a gba jal Sɩpɩr.
44015040	Sɩ Pol or phiir Sɩlasɩ dɩ wɩ jal, sɩ omɩna kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ Kɔ̃tɩn a bɔna wɩ.
44015041	Dɩ le wɩ gba jal Siri na Silisi a cʋʋ we gbɛbɩdarasɔ dɩ wɩ tɩ.
44016001	Agɩpɩ dɩ Pol gba jal Dɛɛrbɩ na Lisitiri, dɩ kpãkpãadaar bɩɛl gɩ a hale dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Timothe; ɔɔ nɩ dʋɔn Juifi khɛrɩkɛ pɩɛrnɩ Thãgba haar, sɩ ɔɔ thɩ do Gɩrɛkɩ.
44016002	Omɩnaakɛ hanɩ Lisitiri na Ɩkɔn n mɩɩrɛ ɔɔda bɔ.
44016003	Dɩ Pol kɔɔ ƴaalɛ a kpaa wɩ ha kha, dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ gbaa a kur khʋ̃ʋ, gɩdonɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ har paarɩle dɩɩ do wɛr fɛʋ jɩrɛ dɩ Gɩrɛkɩ ɔɔ thɩ do.
44016004	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n kpaarnɩ dɩɩra, wɩ-n sor omɩnana wa-n hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ thɔ̃thɔna na we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ gʋʋrnɩ Jerujalɛm.
44016005	Dɩ we gbɛbɩdara n 'lɛr fãga ha pɛrɛra dɩ wɩ jɔrna na pɛr wire wire.
44016006	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuu kɔɔ pɩɛr wɩnɩ wa-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Ajɩra ga, wɩ kpãasɛrɛ Firiji na Galasɩ dɩɩ.
44016007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ thɔɔnɩ Mɩsɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ lõ Bitini, sɩ Jejuu Thu na kɔɔ ha wɩ hʋɛa'.
44016008	Dɩ le wɩ kpãsɛ Mɩsɩ sa dã Tʋrʋasɩ.
44016009	Dɩtɩnɔ Pol kɔɔ yɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɩ̃ yɩr dɩɩ do Masedʋandaar gɩ, a jɩɩlaa da-n bɩɛlɛɛ thakɛ ayɩ: Seere kɛ Masedʋan a taa sɩ.
44016010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol yɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛɛle pɩ, sɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ dapaara kɔrɔ sɩ jal Masedʋan, gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ tue dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn gɩɩkɛ n wɛ sɩnɩ sɩ mɩa le tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ.
44016011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ thenɩ Tʋrʋasɩ, sɩ gbaar bato a jal dẽdẽdẽ Samɔtɩrasɩ, dɩ ga dɩ wɩlla sɩ jal Neapolɩsɩ.
44016012	Dɩ le sɩ kɔɔ gba jal Eilipi dɩɩraakɛ hanɩ Masedʋan caca marara, kolonɩ gɩ kɔɔ do dakha, dɩ sɩ kɔɔ toore dɩɩraale a pʋɔr gbe.
44016013	Hɩɩr wire sɩ kɔɔ ther dɩ khuirə mɩɩr nʋɔra, ka sɩ kɔɔ kpɩɛrnanɩ Thãgba fʋɔr paar na yɩrɛ. Dɩ sɩ kɔɔ toore dɩ sa-n mɩɩna khɛrasɔɔkɛ n gbɛbanɩ kha le.
44016014	Dɩ khɛ bɩɛl hale kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Lidi, a do gbɩlã kẽkẽ ƴaƴabɩdaar, a the Tɩatɩɩr da-n cʋ Thãgba; dɩ a-n pɛr nũu, dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn khɛrʋʋ haar dɩ pɛ nũu gɩrɛraakɛ Pol n sonɩ.
44016015	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ kpɛɛnɩ nyʋɔnɔ na ɔɔ cɔdara pɩ, a kɔɔ bɩɛl sɛr thakɛ ayɩ: Ado sobɔ tibil nɩ-n we mɩ mɔ̃ mɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda, nɩ lona ɩ̃ cɔ a tɔɔ; dɩ a kɔɔ bɩɛl sɛr da-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛna.
44016016	A gele ka pɩ, sɩ jaal Thãgba fʋɔr paar, dɩ thɔ̃daar khɛ bɩɛl gɩ, a hale dɩ sɩ caanaa, dɩ hana Pɩtɔ̃ kɔ̃tɛɛbuukɛ cʋgɛɛnɩ da-n bo, dɩ a-n 'lɛr war jɔɔ ɔɔ borara da-n ha ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ;
44016017	dɩ a mar da-n kpaan Pol na sɛrɛ khiro sɩ da-n hulẽ ayɩ: Tɩbɩlaakɛ Thãgba Kəkəədaarɩ thɔ̃dara wɩ do dɩ wa-n mɩɩ nar taa hʋɛ.
44016018	Wire jɔɔjɔɔ a-n kɔɔ cʋʋ ga thɩ̃ɩlera. Dɩ Pol thʋ̃ vɔɔ a kɛr a so kɔ̃tɛɛbuurəəle ayɩ: Mɩ so farɛ na Jeju Kirisitii i, thɛ khɛrraakɛ. Dɩ the liirrəə dapaara.
44016019	Mɔ̃kɛ thɔ̃daar khɛrɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ yɩɛnɩ dɩ awɩ war 'lɛ hʋ kʋɛrɛ, wɩ fʋrɛ Pol na Sɩlasɩ a hal wɩ jalna tɩɩ jɔ paar kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔ ƴɛra,
44016020	a nɩna so kɩɩldara a so: Tɩbɩlaakɛ nyanyãa sɛr dɩɩ;
44016021	Juifisɔ wɩ do dɩ wa-n mɩɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ sa hananɩ hʋɛ a na tu agɩbo sɩ kpaanɔa', gɩdonɩ Rɔmɛ̃sɔ ha sɩ.
44016022	Dɩ tibil jɔɔle ɩɩrɛ a mana wɩ, dɩ so kɩɩldara so wɩ ɓəəre wi kẽkena sa cile wi na khasa.
44016023	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ bɩɩr wɩnɩ dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ pɩ, wɩ pɛ wɛr khaɩra sa kpãkpãa khaɩ bɛrdaarraakɛ a na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn wɩ.
44016024	Dɩ mɔ̃ khaɩ bɛrdaar nɩɛnɩ thɩmɩɩrɩle, a gba wɛr pɛ khaɩ du thɩ̃thɩɩn sa kpala wɩ nɛɛ na kpulole.
44016025	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ nɩrɔnɩ, Pol na Sɩlasɩ bɩɛlɛ Thãgba dɩ wa-n khɩna nɩɛ dɩ wa-n kpãgana Thãgba, dɩ khaɩdara nɩɛ.
44016026	Dapaara thɩɩ kɔɔ jɩɩn dɩɩ khɩɩr ka, dɩ khaɩ cʋɔr gbugbuyo; dɩ bɔ bɩɛllala loosɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ khɛr, dɩ khaɩdara fɛʋʋ lidasɔ thʋbɩrɛ.
44016027	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ khaɩ bɛrdaar na jaanɩ a yɩ khaɩ loosɔ dɩɩ khɛr, a pher bajɩna a kʋra dɩbara gɩdonɩ a ka jɩna khaɩdara kɔɔ fuulele.
44016028	Sɩ Pol phã nɔ khɩɩr ayɩ: Fa-n cʋʋ afɩ dɩbara puurə', sɩ hakɛ fɛʋ.
44016029	Dɩ khaɩ bɛrdaar bɩɛl dɔɔ a cana birbirbir lõ, a ji Pol na Sɩlasɩɩ ƴɛra da n jẽ kpakpakpa,
44016030	sa kpa wɩ thena a bule wi: Kɔ̃tɩna, anye teana ĩ cʋɛ a 'lɛ taarɛ?
44016031	Dɩ Pol na Sɩlasɩ birsee: Pɩɛr Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn haar dɩ fa 'lɛr taarɛ, fɛrɛ na afɩ cɔdara.
44016032	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ mɩgʋʋrɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ so na wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ ɔɔ cɔ.
44016033	Dɩ a kpa wɛr ga dɩtɩnɔɔlera a thena a cɔcɔɔ wɩ khoisɔ, sɩ dapaara dɩ wɩ kpɛgʋʋ nyʋɔnɔ na ɔɔ cɔdara fɛʋ.
44016034	Dɩ a kpa wɛr a kɔna ɔɔ cɔ a ha wɩ dɩkɔ, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ daaraarɛ kpɛ ɔr na ɔɔ cɔdara fɛʋ mɔ̃ a pɛrnɩ Thãgba haar.
44016035	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ wɩlnɩ, so kɩɩldara thʋɔn gardɛsɔ wɩ jala a sɔ khaɩ bɛrdaarra a faa tɩbɩlaale wɩ kɔ̃.
44016036	Dɩ bɛrdaar gbaar jal a so Polla ayɩ: So kɩɩldara thʋɔn ayɩ, wɩ faa nɩ; gɛr gɩ nɛnɛ̃ nɩ thɛ kɔna na ha ɩɩ.
44016037	Sɩ Pol so gardɛsɔra: Sɛr Rɔmɛ̃sɔɔkɛra wɩ kɔɔ ciilni tibil jɔɔ ƴɛra, sɩ kɩrʋ na yɩr dɩ wɩ jɩ gɩrɛ sɩ cʋʋna', sa to sɩ khaɩra, gɩ do wɩ cʋʋ sɛr dɩ sɩ the thaa waa gbul bɛɛ? Ga ha mã'. Wɛr thɛthɛra n ɩna dɩbara a faa sɩ.
44016038	Dɩ gardɛsɔ gba thɩmɩaale a jalna so kɩɩldarara, dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ mɔ̃ wɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩ Rɔmɛ̃sɔ wɩ do.
44016039	Dɩ wɩ pɔr a phʋʋr wɩ a pɛ wɩ hʋɛra, sa bɩɛl wɩ wɩ thɛ dɩɩra.
44016040	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ thenɩ khaɩra wɩ kɔɔ jaal Lidii pa. A wɩ yɩ omɩna a mɩɩ wɩ ƴɛ kʋʋl jal thɩmɩɩr pɩ, wɩ gbaar kɔ̃.
44017001	Sɩ Pol na Sɩlasɩ kɔɔ kpaarɛ Ãfɩpolɩsɩ na Apolonɩ sa dã Tesalonɩkɩ, ka Juifisɔ hananɩ awɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ.
44017002	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ Pol mɩlna gɩnɩ a lʋʋn le. Dɩ hɩɩr wire yẽther fɛʋ a gbaar Thãgbaa sɛbɛ da-n yɩrna wɩ wɩ yɛ kɩrʋ,
44017003	da-n jɩɩ mɩɛ wɩ da-n nɩna wɩ kɩrʋ, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ teenanɩ Kirisiti n yɩ gaarɛ ɔɔ khi pa sɩ a ɩɩr a the khirera; dɩ a so warɛ Jejuulera dɔ Kirisitiikɛ ɩnɩ-n mɩɩ wɩnɩ.
44017004	Ɩkhasɔ wɛrra jɩrɛ tue dɩ wa-n kpaar kha na Pol, na Sɩlasɩ, na dakha Gɩrɛkɩsɔ bərəəmkɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Thãgba, na khɛ jɔjʋɔɔkɛ jɩɛnnɩ too.
44017005	Sɩ gɩdonɩ gbugi fʋrɛ Juifisɔ, wɩ kpar konaakɛ dɔnɩ ƴatɛ tɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ nɔ ɓaardara, dɩ wɩ ɩɩr a kpa tɩbɩla jɛ sa cʋʋ dɩ wɩ ɩɩr na ɓɔɓɔlɔlɛ dɩɩra. Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ jaal a sɔbɩ Jajɔ̃ɔ cɔ, wɩ ƴaal Pol na Sɩlasɩ, wɩ kpa wɩra wɩ jalna tibil jɔɔ ƴɛra.
44017006	Sɩ gɩdonɩ wa yɩ wa', wɩ kɔɔ kpar Jajɔ̃ na wɩ̃ omisɔ a jalna kɔ̃tɩnaa pa dɩɩra a hulẽ ayɩ: Tɩbɩlaakɛ n fenɩ dɩɩ fɛʋ ɩnɛ kɛ, dɩ Jajɔ̃ tee wɩ.
44017007	Wɛr fɛʋ n kʋɛa Sejaarɩ jɔfʋ dɩ wa-n sona dɩ wɩ yɩ fãgadaar kpɩɩ haleekɛ dɔnɩ Jeju.
44017008	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil jɔɔle na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ nɩɛnɩ thɩmɩɩrɩle, haar ɓʋ̃ɓʋna wɛr.
44017009	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ Jajɔ̃ na wɛ a to helula, sɩ agɩpɩ wɩ faa wɛr dɩ wɩ kɔ̃.
44017010	Dɩ dapaara omɩna cʋʋrɛ Pol na Sɩlasɩ dɩ wɩ ɩɩr kɔrɔ, a the le a jal Bere dɩtɩnɔ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ danɩ le, wɩ kɔɔ lʋʋn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra.
44017011	Wa Juifisɔɔle hananɛ fɩlɛ a jɔ Tesalonɩkɩdara; wɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ na ha bʋɔ, dɩ wɩ 'lo wire fɛʋ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra na hɩɩn, ado gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n so warnɩ otirə gɩ ha.
44017012	Tibil jɔjʋɔɔ wɛrra kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar, na Gɩrɛkɩ khɛrasɔ bərəəmkɛ jɩɛnnɩ too, na konasɔ jɔɔjɔɔ.
44017013	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Tesalonɩkɩ Juifisɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ Pol n mɩɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ dakha Bere, wɩ kɔɔ pɔr a nyanyãa tɩbɩlaa kpɩɛr sa cʋr wɩ a pɛ war.
44017014	Sɩ dapaara omɩna kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ Pol wo dɩ ɩɩr jalna lanyɔ̃ khʋʋ. Sɩ Sɩlasɩ na Timothe toore Bere.
44017015	Sɩ wɩrɛ kɔɔ thɔɔnɩ Pol, Atɛn wɩ kɔɔ danaa sɩ na kɔ̃, dɩ Pol thɔ̃ wɩ wɩ sɔ Sɩlasɩra na Timothera wɩ pɔ kɔrɔ.
44017016	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol toonɩ Atɛn da-n pɩɛr wɩ, haar n heluule mɔ̃kɛ a yɩnɩ thɩla dɩɩ hi dɩɩle.
44017017	Gɛr gɩ dɩ lõ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔra da-n yɩrna Juifisɔ wɩ yɛ kɩrʋ, na dakha wɩrɛɛkɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Thãgba, dɩ ƴatɔɔ dakha mɛ̃ a-n yɩrna wɩrɛɛkɛ a-n caananɩ wire fɛʋ.
44017018	Wɩ̃ thɩ̃ jɩnaakɛ n kpaanɛnɩ Epikuuri too dɩɩrra na Sɩtoyɩsɩɩ too dɩɩrra n mɩɩnaanɛ. Dɩ wɛ na-n so: Anyee thɩmɩɩ ca nɔdadaarɩkɛ n ƴaal a mɩɩ thakɛ? Sɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ nɩɛnɛnɩ da-n mɩɩ Jejuuda na khi ɩɩrɛɛda wɩ sor: Gɩ hor thãgba kpɩɩsɔɔda a-n mɩɩ.
44017019	Dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ kpaa jalna Atɛndaraa so gʋʋr pa, a sʋʋraa: Sɩ punone jɩ dɩɩr phaakɛra fɩ-n dɩɩrnɩɩ kɩr ya?
44017020	Gɩdonɩ sɩ nɩɛrɛ dɩɩr phanaakɛ fɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ, gɛr gɩ dɩ sa-n ƴaal sɩ jɩ kɩrʋ.
44017021	Gɩdonɩ Atɛndara fɛʋ na kpakpalaakɛ hanɩle, awɩda dʋɔn wɩ tɔɔ a na pɛ so phana nũu, agɩbo a na mɩa gɩ dɔrɔɔm.
44017022	Dɩ Pol ɩɩr jɩɩl Atɛndaraa so gʋʋr pa thɩ̃thɩɩn, a so ayɩ: Nɛr Atɛndara, mɩ yɩ nɛr waa dɩ nɩ do thãgba ƴala gel.
44017023	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ mɩ-n kpaarnɩ anɩ dɩra, mɩ yɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ anɩ thɩl ji thɩ̃sɔ; mɩ phurore bonɩ ji pa bɩɛlla dɩɩ khere ayɩ: Thãgbaakɛ tibil na jɩna', ɔr hɩna. Dɩ gɩrɛra nɩ-n fʋɔrnɩ sɩ na jɩ gɩ wa', gɛrra mɩ-n mɩɩ nar gɩrɛ.
44017024	Thãgbaakɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ thɩɩ na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ha garnɩ, ɔrra dɔ Kɔ̃tɩn ƴũ na kɛ thɩɩra, aa-n cɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrraakɛ wɩ mɩnɩ na tibil nyɛ̃a';
44017025	dɩ tibil na puno a na-n dʋʋraa thɔma gɩ ho thɩ̃ɛ n ɓɔraa ga, gɩdonɩ ɔr n 'laanɛ yire na fesue na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
44017026	Ɔr cʋɛ tibil caar fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ tibil bɩɛlɩ məl wɩ hana paar fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ, a kɔɔ mãa pɛrɛ mɔ̃ bɔɔkɛ wa pʋɔrnɩ na hanɩ, na mɔ̃ awɩ cɔ pa pɛl na hanɩ dakha.
44017027	Ɔɔ ƴaal dʋɔn, wa-n ƴaalɛ ɩnɛr Thãgba a dɔ bʋɔ a bəəre phaphapha a yɛ nɩ, sɩrakɛ aa hʋnɔ kha na sɛrɛ bɩɛla'.
44017028	Gɩdonɩ ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sɩ hana yire, ɔr n cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sa-n jal, ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sɩ hakɛ thɩɩra. Mee, mɛ̃ anɩ nɩ pɛdara ɩkhasɔ kɔɔ so ayɩ: “Ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ sɩ do.”
44017029	Dɩ mɔ̃ sɩ donɩ ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ mɛ̃, ga teena sa-n kpɩɛrɛ dɩ mɔ̃ Thãgba hanɩ, a hor thɩlɩkɛ thɩ̃ jɩn n cʋʋnɩ na dɛ, na dɛ bulo, na bokaar mɔ̃ ɔɔ kpɛsɛ hana'.
44017030	Sɩ kpɩɛr 'lee bɔɔle Thãgba na-n therna ga, sɩ nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã a-n sor tɩbɩlala paar fɛʋ dɩ yɩ, wa-n deba haar;
44017031	gɩdonɩ wi bɩɛl hale a dʋnɩ a na gba tibilikɛ a phiirni a kɩɩlna tɩbɩla fɛʋ na fɩl sarʋ, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛra a kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ khirera dɩɩ nɩna tɩbɩla fɛʋ casɩ dɩ thalera ga ha.
44017032	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ da-n mɩɩ khi ɩɩr thɩmɩɩr, ɩkhasɔ n maan, sɩ ɩkhasɔ wer so aa: Dɩkhõo sa bire a na pɛ afɩda nũu wo.
44017033	Mɛ̃ Pol the dɩphã awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
44017034	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ borrakɛ sa maa a pɛr haar, khɛ bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Damarɩsɩ gɩ, na Atɛndaraa so gʋʋrdaar bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Denisi, na wɩ̃ tibil ɩkhasɔ wo.
44018001	A gele pɩ, Pol ther Atɛn a jal Korɛ̃tɩ.
44018002	Dɩ le a caana Juifi kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Akɩlasɩ; Pɔ̃ dɩɩra wɩ kʋ̃ɔ. Ga maan a kɔɔ thenɩ Ɩtalɩ na ɔɔ khɛr Pirisil a pɔa', gɩdonɩ Kʋloodɩ fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ kɔɔ sor Juifisɔra fɛʋ wɩ thɛ Rɔm. Dɩ wɛr Pol n kɔɔ toona.
44018003	Dɩ gɩdonɩ wa kẽkẽ thɔma wɩ-n do, wɩ gbɛbɩrɛ too dɩ wa-n do kha thɔma.
44018004	Hɩɩr wire fɛʋ Pol n gba Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra da-n yɩrna Gɩrɛkɩsɔ na Juifisɔ wɩ pɩɛr haar.
44018005	Dɩ ɔhɔɔkɛ Sɩlasɩ na Timothe kɔɔ thenɩ Masedʋan a pɔ, gɛr Pol jɩɩ tooro Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ togʋʋ waa vʋ̃ʋ, da-n jɩɩ nɩna Juifisɔ dɩ Jeju dʋɔn Kirisiti.
44018006	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Juifisɔ gbɔnaanɩ dɩ wa-n nɩɩrnaa, Pol kpɛɛrɛ thɩlãkobe ɔɔ kẽkena sa so war: A nɩ buur, anɩ so na heen ma', ga 'lɛ ma'. Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã thɩldarara ma-n jal.
44018007	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a thenɩ le a jaal kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Tɩtusi Jusitusii pa, kɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Thãgba. Ɔɔ cɔ, cɔ ɓãa gɩ na Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ.
44018008	Sɩ Kirisipusiikɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra kɔɔ pɛr Kɔ̃tɩn haar na ɔɔ cɔdara fɛʋ. Dɩ Korɛ̃tɩda jɔjʋɔɔkɛ kɔɔ pɛnɩ Polɩ thɩmɩɩ nũu kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar dakha dɩ wɩ kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔ.
44018009	Sɩ dɩtɩnɔ, Kɔ̃tɩn cʋʋrɛ Pol dɩ yɩ thɩ̃ɛ sɩ dɩ sʋʋraa ayɩ: Fa-n do maar n fʋ fa'. Na mɩa ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ, fa-n pɩr pɔba',
44018010	gɩdonɩ mɩ ha kha na fɛrɛ, dɩ tibil na tha far nyɔ̃ɔ a na cʋʋ fɩ puurə'; na mɩa gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla jɔɔ har dɩɩraakɛ, kɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ too.
44018011	Dɩ a toore le yɛ bɩɛl na pora maadõ, da-n dɩɩr Korɛ̃tɩdara Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ.
44018012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Galɩyɔ̃ kɔɔ donɩ gobanɛr Akaɩ dɩɩra, Juifisɔ kɔɔ dor nɔ bɩɛl sa ɩɩrna thɩmɩɩr Polla, a kpaa a jalna kɩɩl paar a so ayɩ:
44018013	Tibilikɛ n tɔr tɩbɩla dɩ pɛr wa-n fʋɔrɛ Thãgba, dɩ ga-n 'li kha kpɩɩ na gɩrɛ jɔfʋ n sona'.
44018014	Dɩ Pol harra nʋɔ a mɩɩ dɩɩ do Galɩyɔ̃ sor Juifisɔra: Adora gɩ hanɩ gɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na sarana' a cʋʋ, agɩbo dɩkhaa thɩ̃ puu gɩ ga dor, ma pɛ nɛr nũu ka nɛr Juifisɔ;
44018015	sɩ ado thɩ̃ banaa gɩ thɩmɩɩrra, na ierasɔ, na anɩ jɔfʋra, nɛr gele ba dɛ; ma ƴaal ɩ̃ do so kɩɩldaar ga thɩnaala';
44018016	sa weele wɩ le kɩɩl paar a faa.
44018017	Dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ fʋ Sɔsɩtɛnɩkɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra a bɩɩr le kɩɩl paar, sɩ Galɩyɔ̃ na therna gɩraka'.
44018018	Dɩ Pol toore Korɛ̃tɩ a pʋɔr; agɩpɩ dɩ fʋɔr omɩna sa gba bato a jal Siri dɩɩra nakha Pirisil na Akɩlasɩ. Sɩ Sãkɩrɛ a kɔɔ bel yʋʋ gɩdonɩ nʋɔ a kɔɔ so.
44018019	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ daan Efɛjɩ; le Pol faa ɔɔ kpãkpãadara sa lõ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra da-n yɩrna Juifisɔ wɩ yɛ kɩrʋ;
44018020	dɩ wɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlʋʋlɛ a tɔɔ a pʋɔrɛ gbe sɩ aa kɔɔ tuə',
44018021	a fʋɔr wɛr sa so ayɩ, gɩ teenanɛ ɩnɩ-n jala fɛtɩraakɛ na hanɩ Jerujalɛm sɩ a Thãgba tu ɩna bire na pɔ; sa gba bato Efɛjɩ a jal.
44018022	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a danɩ Sejare, a gbaar jal Jerujalɛm. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a fʋɔrnɩ we gbɛbɩdara pɩ, a gbaar jal Ãtɩyɔsɩ.
44018023	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a toonɩ Ãtɩyɔsɩ a pʋɔr gbe, a gbaar hʋɛ a jal da-n kpaar Galasɩ a kpaan Firiji a cʋʋ kpãkpãadara fɛʋ dɩ wɩ tɩ.
44018024	Sɩ Juifi bɩɛl gɩ dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Apolɔsɩ, Alesãdɩɩr dɩɩra wɩ kʋ̃ɔ; a dor tɩɩ kpɛsɛɛ a dona Thãgbaa sɛbɛ jɩ kɔ̃tɩn, a pɔ Efɛjɩ.
44018025	Wɩ kɔɔ dɩɩrʋʋrɛ mɔ̃ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋ hanɩ, dɩ mɔ̃ a donɩ tibilikɛ hanɩ phãphãphã, a-n mɩɩrɛ da-n dɩɩrna gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Jejuuda bɔɔbɔɔ; sɩrakɛ Jãa yɔ kpɛɛ a kɔɔ jɩ dɩbara.
44018026	Dɩ a mar da-n mɩɩ na 'lar Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Pirisil na Akɩlasɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ gɩrɛ a-n mɩɩnɩ, wɩ kpaarɛ dɩ wɩ ha kha, dɩ wɩ jɩɩ nɩnaa kɩrʋ mɔ̃ Thãgbaa hʋ hanɩ bɔɔbɔɔ.
44018027	Mɔ̃kɛ a ƴaalnɩ a kpãasɛ a jal Akaɩ, omɩna kɔɔ pɩɛraarɛ 'lar. Dɩ wɩ kherere sɛbɛ a ha kpãkpãadara wɩ teaa. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ danɩ le, a bulle wɩrɛ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ donɩ nɔɔ dɩ wɩ pɛr haar;
44018028	gɩdonɩ a-n punone Juifisɔ thɩ̃ banaana ka tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra, dɩ gba Thãgbaa sɛbɛ da-n nɩna wɩ dɩ Jeju dʋɔn Kirisiti.
44019001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Apolɔsɩ kɔɔ hanɩ Korɛ̃tɩ, gɛr Pol kɔɔ kpaarɔ Ajɩ gɔ̃gɔnana sa dã Efɛjɩ. Dɩ le a caana ɩkhaa kpãkpãadara a bule wi ayɩ:
44019002	Sɩɩ do nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr Thu Phuu ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ pɛrnɩ haar bɛ? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Sa kɔɔ nɩɛ kpɩɩrakɛ dɩ Thu Phuu hala'.
44019003	Dɩ bir bule wi: Sɩ anyee yɔ kpɛɛ ca wɩ kɔɔ kpɛɛ nɩ? Dɩ wɩ birsee: Jãa yɔ kpɛɛ gɩ.
44019004	Dɩ Pol so war: Wɩrɛ debanɩ haar Jã n kɔɔ kpɛɛ nyʋɔnɔ da-n sona war dɩ yɩ, wɩ pɩɛr ʋrɛɛkɛ na kpa narnɩ haar, a thɩɛna gaa Jeju gɩ.
44019005	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ gele, wɩ kɔɔ gbaar Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i a kpɛɛna wɩ nyʋɔnɔ.
44019006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol kɔɔ dɛ̃ɛ warnɩ nyɛ̃ɛ, Thu Phuu kɔɔ gbune a lõ war dɩ wa-n mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩsɔ, dɩ wa-n tinə Thãgba tukɩrʋ.
44019007	Konaale fɛʋ kɔɔ thɔɔrɛ yʋɔr yenyɔ.
44019008	Agɩpɩ Pol kɔɔ lʋʋn Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra da-n mɩɩ na 'lar. Pora yẽther a kɔɔ mɩɩna wɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda, da-n yɩrna wɩ wɩ pɩɛr haar.
44019009	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ ɩkhasɔɔda bonɩ khɩɩr 'lo dɩ wɩ bo ha pɛrɛ, dɩ wa-n mɩɩna thɩmɩɩ puu dɩ wa-n pɛr Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra tibil jɔɔ ƴɛra, Pol faa wɛr sa lee na kpãkpãadara kpɩɩ, sɩ agɩpɩ dɩ jal kũu bɩɛlɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Tɩranusii lakol cɔra da-n yɩrna wɩ wɩ yɛ kɩrʋ.
44019010	Yɛna yenyɔ a kɔɔ cʋʋ, dɩ mɛ̃ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩle Ajɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ Juifisɔ na Gɩrɛkɩsɔ kɔɔ nɩɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩ.
44019011	Dɩ Thãgba har Pol punone da-n cʋʋna nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩna.
44019012	Dɩ wɩ gba ƴɛ pɩɩndaa na kẽkenaakɛ kɔɔ thaanɩ Pol tomɩra, a pɔna na pɛr khodarara; dɩ mɛ̃ khoo n kpɛɛ wɩ dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔla na-n thɩɩr dakha.
44019013	Sɩ wɩ̃ Juifisɔɔkɛ n kpaarɛnɩ mɔlɔ, kɛ dɔnɩ dɔdɔɔdaraakɛ n wɛanɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ n dor bʋɔ, sɩ dɩ wɩ we Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i dɩ wa-n pɛ wɩrɛraakɛ hananɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔla dɩ wa-n so: Mɩ so narɛ, nɩ thɛ na Jejuu iikɛ Pol n gbanɩ da-n mɩɩ.
44019014	Welela n cʋɛnɩ gelela, Sevaakɛ dɔnɩ gbõdaarɩ bikuunsɔ wɛ makonyɔ.
44019015	Dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔl birse wi: Mɩ jɩrɛ Jeju, dɩ Pol dakha mɩ jɩɩrɛ, sɩ nɛrɛ, amɛ nɩ do?
44019016	Sɩ tibilikɛ kɔ̃tɛɛbu hɔ̃hɔlla harɔnɩ ubire a wu war a puno wi fɛʋ, dɩ wɩ caalɛ thɩɩr cʋɔrɔɔle na sãɓɔlɔ̃ na khoisɔ.
44019017	Dɩ Juifisɔ na Gɩrɛkɩsɔɔkɛ hanɩ Efɛjɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛle, dɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩ fɛʋ dɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i kɔɔ dʋbɩrɔrɛ.
44019018	Dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ kɔɔ pɩɛrnɩ haar pɔr a cã so gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ.
44019019	Dɩ wɛ bərəəmkɛ dʋɔnnɩ dɔdɔɔdara, wɩ pɔr na awɩ sɛbɛsɔ, a gbɛbɩ pa bɩɛl a thii tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra. Wɩ therre ga the nɔ dɩɩ thɔɔ war bɔrɔ kpalanyɔ yʋɔr.
44019020	Thale dɔ nɔɔ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩ kɔɔ kpaarnɩ dɩ ga-n pɛr jɔɔ, dɩ gɩ cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ ga do kpãkpalã ga.
44019021	A ga thɩ̃sɔɔle ka pɩ, Pol kpɩɛrɛ hi ɔɔ bɩnɔ sa yɩ, ɩna jaal Jerujalɛm, sɩ Masedʋan ɩna the na Akaɩ sɩ na jal. A sor ayɩ, ado ɩnɩ dã le dɔ ɩnɩ-n yɩ Rɔm dɩɩ dakha.
44019022	Dɩ a thʋɔn ɔɔ bubulsɔ yenyɔ Masedʋan, Timothe na Erasɩtɩ gɩ, sa too Ajɩ gbe.
44019023	Ɔbɔɔlera nyanyaanɛ kɔɔ lʋʋn Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ.
44019024	Kũu bɩɛl gɩ da-n do Demetiriyusi, dɛ bulo phebɩdaar gɩ; ɔr n pheba dɛ bulona dɩɩ do awɩ thɩl cɔ biikɛ hɔnɩ awɩ thɩl khɛr Artemɩsɩɩda, ga-n 'laa khor wa thɔ̃darasɔra kpãkpalã ga.
44019025	Dɩ a kpar wa thɔ̃darasɔra, na wɩrɛ wɩ-n donanɩ kha thɔ̃ bɩɛl a jɛ sa so: Kona, nɩ jɩrɛ ga thɔnaakɛ asɩ thɩ̃ 'lɛ n the,
44019026	dɩ nɩ yɩɛrɛ a nɩɛna dɩ ga do Efɛjɩ dɩɩra gɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ gɩ sɩrɛ fɩɩʋ sɩɩ do Ajɩra fɛʋ gɩ, Pol ʋrɛ n yɩrnanɛ tɩɩ jɔɔ dɩ fi wi na gɩrɛ a-n sonɩ dɩ yɩ, thãgbasɔɔkɛ tibil n cʋʋnɩ na nyɛ̃ɛ na do thãgba bɔsɔa'.
44019027	Sɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ puure, ga do gɩdonɩ asɩ thɔ̃ɔkɛ na debire na do mɔlɔ gɛr gɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ aa: Artemɩsɩ, thɩl khɛ kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛɛ cɔ na do thɩ̃ɛ 'lo bã, dɩrakɛ Artemɩsɩɩkɛ Ajɩdara ɓibi n fʋɔrnɩ na tɩbɩla thɩɩraakɛ fɛʋ aa, ɔɔ i the dakha na kʋɛrɛ koo.
44019028	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ gele, nĩkhii fʋlɛ wɛr dɩ wɩ ma dɩ wa-n hulẽ aa: Efɛjɩdaraa Artemɩsɩ thʋnɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ka.
44019029	Dɩ dɩɩraale koo nyanyaanɛ kɔɔ hale. Dɩ wɩ kha fɛʋ giri a lõ ɓol paarɩle a fʋ Gayʋsɩ na Arɩsɩtarkɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ Masedʋandaraakɛ dɔnɩ dakha Polɩ kpakpaarsɔ.
44019030	Sɩ Pol kɔɔ ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n lõ ɩnɩ-u yɩ tɩbɩlaale, sɩ kpãkpãadara kɔɔ pɩɛrʋʋrɛ.
44019031	Dɩ ɩkha kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ Ajɩdaraakɛ dɔnɩ Polɩ kuunsɔ kɔɔ thʋɔn a sʋʋraa, a na-n lõ ɓol paarɩla'.
44019032	Ɩkhasɔ n hulene dɩ wa-n so awɩda kpɩɩ, wɛ n hulẽ dɩ wa-n so awɩda kpɩɩ, gɩdonɩ gɩ kɔɔ har bʋla bʋla bʋla tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn na jɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ nɔɔ dɩ wɩ kparɔ kha a ja'.
44019033	Dɩ wɩ ti Alesãdɩɩrɩkɛ Juifisɔ tɔnɩ dɩ wa-n pɛr ƴɛ bʋrɔ, dɩ ɩɩr tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thɩɩn da-n jɛ wɩ na nyɛ̃ɛ, a ƴaalɛ a mɩɩ tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃ɛ.
44019034	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ jɩnɩ dɩ Juifi gɩ, wɛr fɛʋ hulene nɔ bɩɛl a pʋɔrna dɩɩ thɔɔ lɩɛr yenyɔ dɩ wa-n so: Efɛjɩdaraa Artemɩsɩ thʋnɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ka.
44019035	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɛbɛ kheredaar punoni tɩbɩla dɩ wɩ pɩr, a sor: Nɛr Efɛjɩdara, ʋmɔ̃ haankɛ na jɩɛnnɩ dɩ Efɛjɩ dɩɩ dʋɔn dɩɩkɛ n hɩnɛnɩ Artemɩsɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ cɔa', na ʋrɛ n hɩnɛnɩ bokaarɩkɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ a ji thɩɩra kɛ n nɛnanɩ dɩ Artemɩsɩ ga.
44019036	Dɩ gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ gɩɩkɛ na hanɩ bana paara' gɩ teenanɛ nɩ pɩra, na-n ɩɩr na cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ thaa birbirə'.
44019037	Gɩdonɩ nɩ kpar tɩbɩlaakɛ a ɩna, sɩ ga do thɩ̃ɛ wɩ kɔɔ yu thɩl cʋɔrɔa', wa kɔɔ kʋɛ dakha wo asɩ thɩl khɛrɩkɛɛ iə'.
44019038	Ado Demetiriyusi na ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔ wɛr hana sor na ntɛ, kɩɩl wire hale dɩ so kɩɩldara dakha hale, dɔ wɩ we kha kɩɩl paar.
44019039	Sɩ ado thɩ̃ kpɩɩ hale dɩ nɩ hana, tɩbɩlaakɛ gobanɛr hanɩ hʋɛ dɩ wɩ kpa na jɛ, wɛr na gʋrɛ gɩ.
44019040	A sa hɩɩna', wa pɛ sarɛ sor khʋɛnaakɛra kɔɔ dananɩ nĩ, gɩdonɩ sa jɩ mɔ̃ sa mɩɩnɩ a na nɩna khʋ̃ɛɛkɛɛ kɩra'.
44019041	A ga thɩmɩɩle pɩ, a bɩlanɛ tɩbɩlaale kpanɩ a jɛ.
44020001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ khʋ̃ɛɛle pɩnɩ, gɛr Pol wer kpãkpãadara a der pa bɩɛl a mɩɩ wɩ wa-n yɩrana ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal, sa fʋɔr wɩ sa gba jal Masedʋan.
44020002	Dɩ a kpaarɛ paarɩle a mɩɩ kpãkpãadara thɩmɩa jɔɔ dɩɩ ha wɩ ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal, agɩpɩ dɩ gba jal Gɩrɛsɩ
44020003	a too le pora yẽther. Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a ƴaalnɩ a lõ bato a jal Siri, a nɩɛrɛ dɩ Jnifisɔ gʋʋrɛ kha sa nʋɔ, dɩ a kpɩɛrɛ a hɩɩn sa bir na Masedʋan hʋɛ a kɔ̃.
44020004	Wɩrɛ kɔɔ thɔgɔɔnɩ ha wɩrɛ: Sopatɛɛrɩkɛ thɛnɩ Bere, Pirusii bikuun gɩ, na Arɩsɩtarkɩ, na Sekɔ̃ɔkɛ thɛnɩ Tesalonɩkɩ, na Gayʋsɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Dɛɛrbɩ, na Timothe, na Tɩsɩkɩ, na Tʋrofɩmɩkɛ wɩ kɔnɩ Ajɩ.
44020005	Wele kɔɔ kʋʋlɛ sɩ ƴɩɛ dɩ wa-n pɩɛr sɩ Tʋrʋasɩ.
44020006	Sɩ se wer, ɔbɔɔkɛ Buruukɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩraa bɔ kanɩ pɩ, gɛr sɩ gbaar bato Filipi, dɩ wire yemɔɩ wire sɩ kɔɔ caan wɛr Tʋrʋasɩ a too le wire makonyɔ.
44020007	Sɩ wire makonyɔɔ caca wi, sɩ kɔɔ kpar kha a jɛ sɩ kho Kɔ̃tɩnɩ dɩko. Sɩ gɩdonɩ, a dɩɩ wɩl gɛr Pol na jaal, a kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ thɩmɩɩr kpãkpãadarara sɩ a mɩɩna wɛr waa dɩ dɩɩ nɩrɔna.
44020008	Dɩ lãphã jɔɔ kɔɔ hale lɩ̃ganaale sɩ-n kpanɩ kha a jɛ.
44020009	Dɩ daɓol bɩɛl gɩ da-n do Etikusi a too fɛnɛtɩrɩra, a daar khi kper ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol mɩɩnɩ thɩmɩa da-n pʋɔrna ƴɛrr, dɩ daan tʋɔrɛ dɩ the le lɩ̃gã yẽtherdaara a təə ji thʋnɔ, dɩ wa gbaa dɩɩ do a khire.
44020010	Sɩ Pol gbune a dɛɛnaa a palʋʋ sa so: Na-n do haar n uu na', gɩdonɩ ɔɔ fesu hale.
44020011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol birni jʋʋn, a khor Kɔ̃tɩnɩ dɩko sa bir fʋ thɩmɩa dɩ dɩɩ wɩlna; agɩpɩ dɩ gba jal.
44020012	Sɩ wɩ kpar daɓolbirile a jalna na yire, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ do warɛ ha faa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ.
44020013	Sɩ se wer, sɩ kɔɔ kʋʋlɛ Pol ƴɩɛ a lõ bato a jal Asɔsɩ, ka sɩ kɔɔ gʋʋrnɩ kha sa caanɛ na gbaa, gɩdonɩ hʋɛ or ƴaal a pɔna.
44020014	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ caan sɩnɩ Asɔsɩ, a lʋʋn batookɛ sɩ harnɩ dɩ sɩ jal Mɩtɩlɛn.
44020015	Le sɩ jal na bato waa, dɩ dɩɩ na wɩl dɩɩ do sɩ daan ka Kɩyɔsɩ dɩɩ pɛnɩ ƴɩɛ. Dɩ ʋ̃ dɩ bir na wɩl dɩ sɩ dã Samɔsɩ, dɩ wireekɛ na kpaanɛnɩ dɩɩ do sɩ daan Mɩle.
44020016	Sɩ Pol kpɩɛrɛ hi ɔɔ bɩnɔ sa yɩ, ɩna kpãasɛrɛ Efɛjɩ sɩ ɩna jɩɩla', dɩ mɛ̃ ɩna dĩdĩə Ajɩ dɩɩra ga; gɩdonɩ a-n phananɛ adora punone hale a dã Jerujalɛm Pãtɩkotɩ wire.
44020017	Sɩ Pol toore Mɩle, sa thɔ̃ Efɛjɩ a we we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ.
44020018	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ pɔnɩ dã a so warɛ ayɩ: A fʋna wireekɛ mɩ lonɩ Ajɩ dɩɩra, nɩ jɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ ɩ̃ fɩl hanɩ bɔɔ fɛʋ na nɛrɛ,
44020019	dɩ ma-n dona Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃ na dɩbara jor koo, nakha yilẽbe, na gaarɛraakɛ mɩ-n yɩnɩ Juifisɔɔ gʋʋrraakɛ wɩ-n gʋʋrnɩ sɩ wa-n nɔ mɩ.
44020020	Nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ ma kɔɔ ker nar thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na bɔ narnɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ-n mɩɩ nɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ dɩ ma-n dɩɩrnanɩ thɩ̃ɛ tibil jɔɔ ƴɛra na cɔnanɔsɔa',
44020021	dɩ mɩ-n kpãkpaanɛ Juifisɔra na wɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa', wɩ deba haar a birə Thãgbara a hanana ha pɛrɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira.
44020022	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ nɩ hɩnɛ, Thu Phuu hala mɩ gɩrɛ da-n jalna Jerujalɛm, sɩ ma jɩ gɩrɛ na dana mɩnɩ la';
44020023	sɩ gɩrɛ mɩ jɩnɩ dɩbara dʋɔn: Dɩɩ wo dɩɩraakɛ mɩ-n kpaarnɩ, Thu Phuu n nɩ marɛ dɩ khaɩ lʋʋn na bɔ gaarɛ n hale dɩ ga-n pɩɛr mɩ.
44020024	Sɩ ma-n ɩherna ĩ yi dɩɩ do mar thɩ̃ ɓʋ̃ɔa', sɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ dʋɔn ado mɩ puno pɩ ɩ̃ kɔlɔ̃kɔɔ ca na dakha thɔmaakɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ha mɩnɩ ayɩ, ɩ̃ mɩa Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ.
44020025	Dɩ nɩ hɩnɛ nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã, na yɩ mɩ ƴɛ bire bã nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ kɔɔ kpaarɔnɩ a mɩɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda.
44020026	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ma-n so nar nĩ gɩrɛ casɩ, ado nɩ buu anɩ so na heen ma',
44020027	gɩdonɩ mɩ mɩɩ nɛr gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa ƴaal fɛʋ sɩ ma ker nar dɩkha ga.
44020028	A nɩ jɩ na-n dɔ bʋrɛ anɩbara na banaa fɛʋʋkɛ Thu Phuu kɔɔ pɛ narnɩ nɩ dɔrɔ hɩɩndara ayɩ, na-n khɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ a kɔɔ thenɩ na ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ tɔmɩ̃.
44020029	Mɩ jɩrɛ a mɩ kɔ̃ na pɩ, kpe hɔ̃hɔla na lʋʋn anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn dɩ wa sɩ banaanaaka';
44020030	wo, tɩbɩla na ɩɩrɛ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn wa-n dɩɩr thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ gõgolonenɩ wɩ kɛr kpãkpãadara wa-n kpa war.
44020031	Gɛr gɩ na-n jʋrɛ a jɛna gɩ, dɩ yɛna yẽther biləni mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ, sɩ ma-n kɔɔ sɩrɔ fɩl dɩɩrɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛlla na yilẽbe dɩtɩnɔ na dɩwɩlʋa'.
44020032	Dɩ nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã Kɔ̃tɩnɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ mɩ faa nɩ na ɔɔ bɔ jɩ thɩmɩɩra, kɛ hananɩ punone a na cʋʋ nɩ dɩ na khɔ̃, kɛ na hana nɩnɩ dakha anɩdaakɛ na hɩnɩ na wɩrɛ Thãgba leenɩ kpɩɩ.
44020033	Ma kɔɔ ƴaal tibillə war, dɩ dɛ gɩ, dɩ kẽkena ga.
44020034	Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ jɩrɛ dɩ mɩ-n dor thɔma na ɩ̃ nyɛ̃ɛkɛ, dɩ ma-n 'lɛ gɩrɛ n ɓɔra mɩnɩ nakha wɩrɛɛkɛ n kɔɔ hana mɩnɩ kha.
44020035	Dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra mɩ kɔɔ nɩ narɛ na-n dɔ thɔma thale a na bulo wɩrɛ yɔɔnɛnɩ, a na jɛnana Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ sonɩ ayɩ: 'Laarɛ n hananɛ Thãgba bɔnanɛ dɩɩ jɔ 'lɛr.
44020036	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a mɩɩnɩ thale pɩ, a gulẽgarɛ dɩ wɩ bɩɛl kha Thãgba fɛʋ.
44020037	Dɩ wɛr fɛʋ n khɩɩrɛ wɛlɛ wɛlɛ wɛlɛ a palna Pol dɩ wa-n fʋɔrʋʋ
44020038	sa gbobi; sɩ gɩrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ so warnɩ ayɩ, wa yɩ nɩ ƴɛ bire bã dɔ war sor. Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ thɔgʋʋrɛ a dana bato.
44021001	Sɩ sɛrɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ leenɩ kha, sɩ gbaar bato a jal dẽdẽdẽ Kɔsɩ; a dɩɩ wɩl sɩ jaal Rɔɔdɩ a the le a jal Patara.
44021002	Dɩ mɔ̃ sɩ yɩnɩ bato bɩɛlɩkɛ na jalanɩ Fenɩsɩ, sɩ lʋʋn a jal
44021003	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ 'laanɩ yɩ Sɩpɩr yɔ dɩɩ, sɩ faa gɛr nyɔ̃bɩlana sa gba asɩ hʋ a jalna Siri khʋʋ a dã Tɩɩr; liir wɩ tiir thɩ̃ɛsɔ batora.
44021004	Dɩ sɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ kpãkpãadara a too le wire makonyɔ. Dɩ kpãkpãadara sor Polla dɩɩ do Thu Phuu pa gɩ the ayɩ, a na-n jal Jerujalɛmna ga.
44021005	A wiresɔɔle ka pɩ, sɩ ɩɩrɛ a gba asɩ kpaar pa hʋ, dɩ kona fɛʋ, na khɛra, na bɩsana kɔɔ thɔɔ sɛr a thena dɩ khuirə. Dɩ sɩ kɔɔ gulẽgarɛ le lanyɔ̃ gẽgerẽ nʋɔra a bɩɛl Thãgba.
44021006	Agɩpɩ dɩ sɩ fʋɔr kha bɩɛlbɩɛl sa lõ batora, sɩ wɛr wɩ kɛrrɛ bir awɩ cɔ.
44021007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ thenɩ Tɩɩr, sɩ gbaar asɩ hʋ a jal dã Pʋtolemaɩsɩ, liir asɩ kpaar lanyʋɔnna khu, dɩ le sɩ bule kha bɔɔ na omɩna sa too kha wi bɩɛl.
44021008	A dɩɩ wɩl sɩ kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ jal Sejare a lõ Filipiikɛ dɔnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩdaarɩ cɔ, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ tibil bɩɛl tɩbɩla makonyɔraakɛ wɩ kɔɔ phiirni, dɩ le sɩ cɔ.
44021009	A hananɛ bikhɛna yenãakɛ na kɔɔ jɛnɩ kona pa', dɩ wa-n ti Thãgba tukɩrʋ.
44021010	Mɔ̃ sɩ toonɩ le a na pʋɔr, Thãgba tukɩr tidaar bɩɛl hale dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Agabusi, Jude a the
44021011	a pɔ asɩ pa; dɩ a gbaar Polɩ lophɛrɛ a linə ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ nɛ na nyɛ̃ɛ sa so ayɩ: Thu Phuu sor aa: Kuunikɛ hɩnanɩ lophɛrɛɛkɛra, thakɛ Juifisɔ na fʋʋ na li Jerujalɛm dɩɩra a na ha ca kpala.
44021012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ nɩɛnɩ gele, sɛrɛ na wɩrɛ hanɩ paarɩlera kɔɔ phʋʋrɛ Pol a na-n jal Jerujalɛmnana ga.
44021013	Dɩ le a birse: Anye nɩ-n cʋʋrɔ thaa dɩ na-n khɩɩ dɩ haar kʋɛ mɩ? Gɩdonɩ mɩ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ, ga do wɩ to mɩ khaɩra dɩbara ga, sɩ dɩ ma khi Jerujalɛm, gɩ do Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i dɔ nɔɔ.
44021014	Dɩ mɔ̃ aa-n ƴaalnɩ a tuə', sa kɔɔ bir jalna gɩ ƴɔɔ bã sɩ sɩ sor: Dɩ dɔ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ tuur n cʋʋ.
44021015	A ga wisɔɔle ka pɩ, sɩ gbɛbɩrɛ asɩ thɩ̃sɔ sɩ jal Jerujalɛm.
44021016	Dɩ wɩ̃ kpãkpãadaraakɛ dɔnɩ Sejaredara kɔɔ thɔɔ sɛr a jalna Manasɔ̃ɔ cɔ kãkɛ gɩ teenanɩ sɩ tɔɔ; tibil gɩɩkɛ wɩ kɔnɩ Sɩpɩr yɔ dɩɩra, a kɔɔ mãa dʋʋr kpãkpãadaar.
44021017	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ danɩ Jerujalɛm, omɩna kɔɔ tee ser na daʋ.
44021018	A ga dɩ wɩl, Pol kpa sɛr a jalna Jakɩɩ cɔ, kãkɛ we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ fɛʋ kpanɩ kha a jɛ.
44021019	A sɩ fʋɔr wɩ pɩ, a mar da-n mɩɛ wɩ dɩɩdɩɩ thɔmaakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ cʋʋnaanɩ ca kpalaa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
44021020	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ gele, wɩ-n dʋbɩrɛ Thãgbaa i; agɩpɩ dɩ wɩ sʋʋraa: Asɩ omi, fɩ yɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ Juifisɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃ pɛrnɩ haar, dɩ wɛr fɛʋ n pərre jɔfʋra.
44021021	Wɩ-n yɩ aa, mɔ̃ fɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ Juifisɔ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ ca kpalaa thɩ̃thɩɩn fɩ-n yɩ, wɩ faa Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ dɩ fɩ sona war dakha aa, wa-n kur bɩsana khʋ̃a', wa-n hɩɩn dakha mama fɩla'.
44021022	Mɔ̃ sa do gɩrɛ, gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na nɩɛrɛ dɩ fɩ ɩnɛ kɛ.
44021023	Gɛr gɩ, cʋɛ gɩrɛ sa so farnɩ: Tɩbɩla yenã hakɛ asɩ pa a so nʋɔ.
44021024	Kpa wɩ nɩ phʋɔl kha, sa lɩma gɩrɛ wa kɔɔ kʋɛnɩ sɩ wɩ puno wɩ bel yʋʋ. Dɩ mɛ̃ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na jɩ dɩ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ dɩ wɩ mɩɩ dɩ wa-n pɛ far, sõsor gɩ, sɩ fɛrɛ dakha fa-n jɩɩ ɩɩr bɔɔbɔɔ fa-n hɩɩnna jɔfʋ.
44021025	Sɩ ado ca kpalaakɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar gɩ, sɩ kɔɔ gʋʋrɛ hɩɩn sa yɩ, wɩ bɔ bonɩ ji nʋʋn, na tɔmɩn, na nʋmɩkɛ khenɩ sɩ tɔmɩn na tha', na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ.
44021026	Dɩ Pol kpar konaale dɩ wɩ phʋɔl kha, dɩ dɩɩ wɩl dɩ wɩ lõ kha Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna wɩ so tɩbɩlala wireekɛ awɩ phʋɔl na pɩnɩ, na ɔbɔɔkɛ wa jini bonɩɛ a na pɛ war fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
44021027	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wire makonyɔɔle n thɔɔnɩ pɩr, Juifisɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Ãjɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ Pol Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, a tɔ tibil jɔ a pɛr dɩ wɩ fʋʋ,
44021028	sɩ wa-n hulẽ: Ɩjɩrayɛldara, nɩ ɩna a bulo si. Ʋrɛ dɔ kuunikɛ n dɩrɛnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ da-n kpaarna paar fɛʋ da-n kpɛna tɩbɩla, na jɔfʋ, na paarɩkɛ. A kparrakɛ Gɩrɛkɩsɔ a lona Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ a ƴɔ̃ƴɔɔna pa phuukɛ.
44021029	Gɩdonɩ wi bɩɛl wɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ Tʋrofɩmɩkɛ dɔnɩ Efɛjɩdaar dɩɩra nakha ɔr, a ka jɩna Pol kpaarɛ a lona Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ.
44021030	Dɩ dɩɩ fɛʋ tutugore, dɩ tɩbɩla na-n caalɛ dɩɩdɩɩ. Dɩ wɩ fʋrɛ Pol Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ, a hal thena sa khaan loosɔ dapaara.
44021031	Mɔ̃ wɩ n ƴaalnɩ wɩ kʋʋ, tutugore daan sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ dɩ nyanyaanɛ har Jerujalɛm dɩɩra fɛʋ.
44021032	Dɩ dapaara dɩ kpa sɔrasɛ na sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, a cana pɔna. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩnɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ na sɔrasɛsɔ wa-n be Pol bã.
44021033	Dɩ le sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ dã a fʋʋ sa so, wɩ lie na jɔrkɔ yenyɔ sa bulee ntɛ a donɩ na gɩrɛ a cʋʋnɩ.
44021034	Sɩ tibil jɔɔlee thɩ̃thɩɩn, wɛ n hulene dɩ wɩ yɩ aa: Gɩrɛ gɩ; wɛ n hulẽ aa: Thakɛ gɩ; sɩ mɔ̃kɛ aa punoni na jɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ sobɔra' gɩdonɩ khʋ̃ɛ jɔrɛ, a sor wɩ kpaa a jalana sɔrasɛɛ cɔ.
44021035	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol kɔɔ danɩ jʋʋn paar, sɔrasɛ thar thʋnɔ sa gbaa, gɩdonɩ nĩkhii thʋnɛ fʋlɛ tɩbɩlaale ka ɔrra.
44021036	Gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla bərəəm n kpaanɛ dɩ wa-n hulẽ aa, wɩ dɔ kuunikɛ n khi.
44021037	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ hanaanɩ wa-n lona sɔrasɛɛ cɔ, Pol bulele sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ aa: Mɩ hananɛ hʋɛ a na so far thɩ̃ɛ ya? Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ birsee: Fɩ-n nɩrɛ gɩrɛkɩ thɩmɩɩr ya?
44021038	Ga do fɛr dɔ Ejipitidaarɩkɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnanɩ lãʋ kɩɛr delẽ delẽ, a kpana tɩɩ kʋdara gbɩlanɩ yenã a jalna bəənnə gaa?
44021039	Dɩ Pol birsee: Mɛrɛ, Juifi ha mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ the Silisi, Tarsɩ dɩɩraakɛ na hanɩ gbə' wɩ kɔ̃ mɩ; mɩ-n bɩɛl fɛr, ha mɩ hʋɛ ɩ̃ mɩɩna tɩbɩlaakɛ.
44021040	Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ haa hʋɛ, dɩ Pol ɩɩr jɩɩl jʋʋn paar sa jɛ tɩbɩla na nyɛ̃ɛ. Dɩ wɩ pɩrrɛ dĩi, dɩ Pol gba thɩmɩa na ebirə thɩmɩɩr da-n mɩɩ wɩ ayɩ:
44022001	Nɛr omɩna na thɛsɔ, nɩ pɛ nũu ĩ so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ thɩmɩɩraakɛ mɩ hananɩ nɛnɛ̃.
44022002	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ nɩɛnɩ da-n mɩɩna wɩ ebirə thɩmɩɩr, wɩ jɩɛ pɩr dɩphã cɩcɩcɩ. Dɩ Pol so war:
44022003	Juifi ha mɩ, Silisi Tarsɩ wɩ kɔ̃ mɩ, sɩ kɩɛr dɩɩraakɛ wɩ kɔɔ haan mɩ, dɩ Gamalɩɛlɩ kal ƴɔɔ mɩ kɔɔ too a dɩɩr thɩ̃ɛ a jɩ mɔ̃kɛ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ jɔfʋ hanɩ ɓibi. Mɩ-n kɔɔ gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛ Thãgbaadara mɔ̃kɛra nɛrɛ fɛʋ hanɩ gɩrɛ nĩ.
44022004	Mɩ kɔɔ kpoore wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋraakɛ, dɩ ma n kʋʋrna wɩ, dɩ ɩ̃ fʋlɛna kona na khɛra a li a na to khaɩra.
44022005	Gbõdaar na kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔkɛ punone mɩɩ nɩ ɩ̃da mɔ̃ gɩ hanɩ. Wɛr thɛthɛrarakɛ mɩ kɔɔ tee sɛbɛ ɩ̃ jalnana ɩ̃ ha omɩnaakɛ hanɩ Damasɩ, sɩ ɩ̃ fʋlɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ hanɩle ɩ̃ ɩnana Jerujalɛm ɩ̃ heen wɩ sor.
44022006	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ hʋɛra dɩ ma-n wɔrɔ̃ Damasɩ, ʋlkhɔɔ gɩ kɔɔ do, dɩ dapaara dahɩrɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ kɔɔ ther ƴũ a carã dii mar;
44022007	dɩ ɩ̃ təə ji thʋnɔ sa nɩɛ wire dɩɩ so mar aa: Sɔl, Sɔl, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa-n kpoo mar mɛ̃?
44022008	Dɩ ɩ̃ birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, fɛr amɛ gɩ? Dɩ birse mi: Mɛr dʋɔn Najarɛtɩ Jejuukɛra fɩ-n kpooronɩ.
44022009	Wɩrɛ kɔɔ hanɩ kha na mɛrɛ wɩ yɩrɛ dahɩrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ, sɩ wa kɔɔ nɩ wireekɛ mɩana mɩna'.
44022010	Dɩ le mɩ bulee, ɩ̃ cʋɛ anye ya, Kɔ̃tɩn? Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn birse mi ayɩ, ɩ̃ ɩrɛ jala Damasɩ; le wa so mar gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba thɩɩn marnɩ ɩ̃ cʋɛ.
44022011	Sɩ gɩdonɩ dahɩrɛ caranɛɛle cʋʋ mɛr dɩ ma-n ya', wɩrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ hana mɩnɩ kha fʋ mɛr nyɔ̃ɔ a hal dɩ ɩ̃ dã Damasɩ.
44022012	Sɩ kũu bɩɛl gɩ da-n do Ananɩasɩ; a-n cʋrɛ Thãgba da-n hɩɩnna ɔɔ jɔfʋ, dɩ Juifisɔ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ dɩɩraale n mɩɩrɛ ɔɔda bɔ,
44022013	a pɔr a jɩɩl mar sa so mar: Sɔl ɩ̃ omi, birə na yɛ. Dɩ liirrə dapaara ɩ̃ yi khɛr dɩ ɩ̃ yɩɩ.
44022014	Dɩ so: Asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ Thãgba thɩnɛ fɩ fɩ jɛ ɔɔ tuur, a yɛ Tɩɩ sarʋ, a nɛ ɔɔ nɔ thɩmɩɩ;
44022015	gɩdonɩ fɛr na dɔ ʋrɛ na-n mɩanɩ ɔɔda tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra, mɔ̃kɛra fɩ yɩɛnɩ a nɩɛna dɩɩ ha.
44022016	Dɩ nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã, anye sɛ fɩ 'lo? Ɩrɛ, wɩ kpɛɛ fɩ nyʋɔnɔ, dɩ dɔ dakha afɩ sopugo n cɔcɔɔ mɔ̃ fɩ wenɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i.
44022017	Dɩ mɔ̃ mɩ kɛrnɩ bir dã Jerujalɛm dɩ ma-n bɩɛl Thãgba Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, mɩ yɩrɛ thɩ̃ yɩr dɩɩ do daphuronaa.
44022018	Kɔ̃tɩn mɩ yɩ dɩ so mar ayɩ: Phana kɔrɔ a thɛ Jerujalɛm, gɩdonɩ wa tu ɩ̃daakɛ fa mɩɩnɩ a na pɛ mara'.
44022019	Dɩ ɩ̃ so: Kɔ̃tɩn, wɛr thɛthɛ jɩrɛ dɩ mɛr n kɔɔ fʋlɛnɛ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ wɩrɛ kɔɔ pɛ fɩnɩ haar dɩ ɩ̃ ciil, sa to wɩ khaɩra.
44022020	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n kʋnɩ Etɩɛn afɩ sobɔ so jɩdaar, mɩ kɔɔ harrɛ a tu awɩda dɩ ma-n hɩɩn wɩrɛ n kʋɔnɩɩ kẽkẽsɔ.
44022021	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn so marɛ ɩ̃ jala aa, ƴɔɔ ɩna thɔ̃ mɩ ca kpalaa pa.
44022022	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ nũu phaphapha a dana thɩmɩɩrɩle sa hulẽ ayɩ: Cʋɛ tibil ca ʋrɛ a khi, aa teena yi hara'.
44022023	Dɩ wɩ hulene dɩ wa-n dʋʋrna kẽkena, dɩ wɩ kpɩɩrna thɩn na dʋʋrna ƴũ.
44022024	Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ sor wɩ kpa Pol a lonana sɔrasɛɛ cɔ a ciilee na khasa sa bulenee, a jɛ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɩrʋ dɩ wɩ hulẽ thale na pɩɛraa.
44022025	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ liini na lɔ pɩ sɩ wɩ ciil, a bulele sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ jɩlɛnɩ bɛrrɔ ayɩ: Nɩ hananɛ hʋɛ na ciil kuunikɛ dɔnɩ Rɔmɛ̃ na khasa, kɛ wa heennɩnakɛ sora ya?
44022026	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ nɩɛnɩ gele, a jaal so sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋra: Mɔ̃ fa do gɩrɛ? Kuunikɛ Rɔmɛ̃ gɩ.
44022027	Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ pɔr a so Polla: Sɔ mar Rɔmɛ̃ ha fɩ gerɩ? Dɩ birsee: Ɔɔ.
44022028	Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ bir so: War mer kʋɛ jɔɔ sa debi a do gɩ. Dɩ Pol birsee, sɩ me wer mɛ̃ wɩ kɔɔ kɔ̃ mɩ.
44022029	Dɩ dapaara wɩrɛ kɔɔ gbɛbanɩ pɩ wɩ ciil Pol, wɩ fagʋʋrɛ; dɩ mɔ̃ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ do Rɔmɛ̃ Pol do, maar fʋʋrɛ gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ liire.
44022030	A dɩɩ wɩl, sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ ƴaalɛ a jɩɩ jɩ bɔɔbɔɔ gɩrɛra dɔnɩ kɩrʋ dɩ Juifisɔ pɩɛraa sor; a thʋbʋʋrɛ sa we bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na so gʋʋrdara fɛʋ, dɩ wɩ kpa kha a jɛ sɩ dɩ kpaa gbuno awɩ ƴɛra.
44023001	Sɩ Pol na-n hɩɩn so gʋʋrdara kirkirkir sa so: Omɩna, ɩ̃ fɩlɩkɛ mɩ hananɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ na hana sɩ paara'.
44023002	Dɩ Ananɩasɩ gbõdaar so wɩrɛraakɛ wɔrɔnɛɛnɩ aa, wɩ bɩɛ nʋɔra.
44023003	Dɩ Pol sʋʋraa: Thãgba na be fer, fɛrkɛ hɔnɩ go biseekɛ wɩ calnɩ mɩlɛ. Fɩ ka toore fa-n kɩɩlna mɩ mɔ̃ jɔfʋ sonɩ, sɩɩ do jɔfʋ fɩ ka fa-n kʋɛ a 'laa hʋɛ wɩ bɛ mɩ.
44023004	Dɩ wɩrɛ wɔrɔnaanɩ sʋʋraa: Thãgbaa gbõdaar fɩ nɩɩrɩɩ?
44023005	Dɩ Pol so: Omɩna, ma kɔɔ jɩ dɩ gbõdaar ga, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: Fa-n mɩɩ puure afɩ tibilsɔɔ kɔ̃tɩna ga.
44023006	Mɔ̃ Pol jɩnɩ dɩ tɩɩ jɔɔle wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala' har kho bɩɛl, jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara kho bɩɛl, a hulene so gʋʋrdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn aa: Omɩna, jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar ha mɩ, dɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara kɔna mɩ, nũu pɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ hananɩ khi ɩɩrɛra dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ wa-n kɩɩlna mɩ gɩrɛ.
44023007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a sonɩ gele, thɩ̃ banaa kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdarara na wɩrɛraakɛ n yɛnɩ khi ɩɩrɛ na hala', dɩ tibil jɔɔle lee kha.
44023008	Gɩdonɩ Sadʋsɛ̃ɛsɔ n yɩ: Khi ɩɩrɛ na hale, dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu gɩ, dɩ thue ga; sɩɩ do jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara wer n ture gelela fɛʋ.
44023009	Dɩ khʋ̃ɛ ɩɩr dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, dɩ ɩkhaa jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaraakɛ dɔnɩ bɩɛl na jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdara ɩɩrɛ, a lã dɩɩ khɩɩr ka sa yɩ: Sa yɩ puure kuunnaaka'; agakpaana gɩ do thue, agɩbo thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ mɩanaa.
44023010	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ khʋ̃ɛ bonɩ dɩ a-n pɛr, maar fʋrɛ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ dɩ kpɩɛr agakpaana tɩbɩlaale na cɛcɛbɛrɛ Pol. Dɩ a sor sɔrasɛra wɩ jala a taa Pol awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a lonanaa sɔrasɛɛ cɔ.
44023011	Ga dɩtɩnɔɔlera, Kɔ̃tɩn pɔr a jɩɩl Pol gɛllɔ sa sʋʋraa: Pɩɛr 'lar, gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ fɩ mɩɩnɩ ɩ̃ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr Jerujalɛm dɔ fɩ mɩɩ gɩ mɛ̃ dakha Rɔm dɩɩra.
44023012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ wɩlnɩ, Juifisɔ n gʋʋrɛ kha sɩ wɩ nɔ Pol a ʋlfɛ awɩbara ayɩ, dɩkor na lõ nɩ nɔɔ dɩ nyʋɔn ga phaphapha ɩnɩ-n kʋʋ.
44023013	Wɩrɛ kɔɔ gʋʋrɛnɩ kha wɩ nʋɔ, wɩ kar tɩbɩla kpalanyɔra;
44023014	dɩ wɩ jaal a yɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ a so war: Sɩ ʋlfɛrɛ ʋlfɛrɛ a pɛ asɩbara ayɩ: Dɩkor na lõ sɩ nɔa' phaphapha sɩ kʋ Pol.
44023015	Gɛr gɩ nɛrɛ dakha nɛnɛ̃kɛ, nɩ dɔ bɩɛl na so gʋʋrdara sa so sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋra a kpaa a ɛna anɩ ƴɛra, gɩ ho nɩ-n jɩɛ ƴaal nɩ gʋʋr ɔɔ sora bɔɔbɔɔ; sɩ sɛrɛ, sɩ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ sɩ kʋʋ sɩ a na dã kɛ pa'.
44023016	Sɩ Polɩ õkhɛrɩ bikuun kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ wɩ gʋʋrnɩ sɩ wɩ nʋɔ, a jal sɔrasɛɛ cɔ a lõ a so Polla.
44023017	Dɩ Pol we sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl a sʋʋraa: Kpa daɓolbirikɛ a jalana sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋra, gɩdonɩ a hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ a na sʋʋraa.
44023018	Dɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ kpa daɓolbirile a jalna sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋra a sʋʋraa: Pol khaɩdaar kɔɔ we mer a bɩɛl mɩ ɩ̃ kpa daɓolbirikɛ a ɛna far aa: A hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ a na so far.
44023019	Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋʋle fʋ daɓolbirile nyɔ̃ɔ a kpaa kana pa kpɩɩ, a bulee: Anye fɩ hana dɩ fa-n so mar?
44023020	Dɩ birsee: Juifisɔ kɔɔ gʋʋrɛ kha, sɩ ɩnɩ-n bɩɛl fɩ fɩ kpa Pol fɩ pɔna cʋɔ so gʋʋrdaraa ƴɛra, gɩ ho thɩ̃ɛ fɩ-n ƴaal fɩ jɩɩ bulee bɔɔbɔɔ.
44023021	Fa-n pɛ wɩ nũə', gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla kpalanyɔ na dɛbɩrɛ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn nɔr dɩ wa-n pɩɛrʋʋ; wɩ kɔɔ ʋlfɛrɛ a pɛ awɩbara ayɩ, dɩkor na lõ nɩ nɔɔ dɩ nyʋɔn ga phaphapha ɩnɩ-n kʋ Pol; wɩ gbɛbɩrɛ gɩrɛ pɩ sɩɩ do afɩ tuur wɩ-n pɛ nũu.
44023022	Dɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ faa daɓolbirile a kɔna sa sʋʋraa, a na n so tibillə dɩ a mɩɛ nɛr thɩ̃ɛɛla'.
44023023	Dɩ le sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ we sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ yenyɔ a so war ayɩ: Nɩ gbɛbɩrɛ a te sɔrasɛ taanyɔ, na sɔrasɩ gãgodara kpalãther yʋɔr, na kpɩladara taanyɔ, nɩ jal Sejare phɩɩn bɔɔ.
44023024	A sor, wɩ hana Pol dakha gãgʋʋsɔɔkɛ a na jʋʋnnɩ, wɩ kpaa pɔlpɔlpɔl wɩ jalna Felɩsɩ gobanɛrɩ pa.
44023025	Dɩ a kherere sɛbɛ thakɛ ayɩ:
44023026	Mɛr, Kʋloodɩ Lɩjɩasɩ khera sɛbɛɛkɛ fɛr Felɩsɩ gobanɛr bʋɔra, dɩ ma-n ha fɩ fʋɔrɛ.
44023027	Kuunikɛ Juifisɔ fʋɔnɛɛ wɩ kʋra, sɩɩ do mɩ pɔnanɛ sɔrasɛsɔ a tagʋʋ na pɩ gɩdonɩ mɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ Rɔmɛ̃ a do.
44023028	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ jɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɩrʋ dɩ wɩ pɩɛraa sor; gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ kpaa a jalna awɩ so gʋʋrdarasɔɔ ƴɛra.
44023029	Dɩ le mɩ yɩɛ dɩɩ do sorɩkɛ wɩ-n pɩɛraanɩ, awɩ jɔfʋ gɩ-n hɩɩn, sɩɩ do aa cʋʋ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ kɛ teananɩ khir dɩ khaɩ tʋʋr ga.
44023030	Mɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dakha dɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ gʋʋrɛ kha sɩ wɩ nʋɔ; gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ thɔnaa dapaara sa so ɔɔ so pɛdarara wɩ pɔ far le a pɩɛraa sorra. Nɩ tɔɔ bɔɔ.
44023031	Mɛ̃ sɔrasɛsɔ kpa Pol dɩtɩnɔ a jalna Ãtɩpatɩrɩsɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ kɔɔ so warnɩ.
44023032	A dɩɩ wɩl, wɩ sɩrɛ sɔrasɩ gãgodarara wɩ kpaa jalana, sa kɛr bir sɔrasɛɛ cɔ.
44023033	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɔrasɩ gãgodara danɩ Sejare, wɩ gbaar sɛbɛɛle a ha gobanɛr a kpana Pol dakha a haa.
44023034	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ gobanɛr hɩɩnnɩ sɛbɛɛle pɩ, a bulele Pol dɩ ʋrɛra a thenɩ; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a jɩnɩ dɩɩ do Silisi a the,
44023035	a sʋʋraarɛ ayɩ: Ado afɩ so pɛdarasɔ ɩ̃, gɛr ma bule far thɩ̃ɛ. Sɩ a sor wa-n hɩnɛɛ Ɛrɔɔdɩɩ cɔ kɔ̃tɩna.
44024001	A wire yemɔɩ ka, Ananɩasɩ gbõdaar pɔr na wɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, na kuunikɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Tɛrtul, kɛ n heenenɩ tɩbɩla sor mɔ̃ awɩ jɔfʋ hanɩ. Dɩ wɩ pɛrɛ Pol sor gobanɛrɩ yɛra.
44024002	Dɩ wɩ wer Pol, dɩ pɔ dã dɩ Tɛrtul ma da-n pɩɛraa sor thakɛ ayɩ: Felɩsɩ bʋɔ, fɛr n cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sɩ toona ha ie bʋɔ; afɩ kpɛsɛ thɔ̃ɔkɛ fɩ donɩ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ thɩ̃ɛ bir debi dɩphã a bɔr asɩ cara.
44024003	Sɩ-n fʋɔr fɛr ka gɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ sɩ-n 'lɛnɩ thakɛ paar fɛʋ.
44024004	Sa-n ƴaal sɩ vɔɔ fa', gɛr gɩ sɩ-n bɩɛl fɛr pɛ sɩ nũu bɔɔ fɩɩʋ gɩrɛraakɛ sɩ hananɩ sɩ so far, gɩdonɩ tɩɩ bʋɔ fɩ do.
44024005	Sɩ yɩrɛ kuunikɛ dɩɩ do khaakhaardaar gɩ; ɔr n ɩrɛna nyanyaanɛ Juifisɔra fɛʋ thɩɩra ɓibi, ɔr dʋɔn dakha kɔ̃tɩn wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ Najarɛtɩdara awɩ ƴɛra kpɩɩ.
44024006	Dɩ a kɔɔ ƴaalɛlakɛ dakha a ƴɔ̃ƴɔ̃ɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, gɛr gɩ dɩ sɩ fʋʋ. [Dɩ sɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛla sɩ kɩɩlnaa mɔ̃ asɩ jɔfʋ hanɩ.
44024007	Sɩ Lɩjɩasɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ pɔr a taa sar na fãga,
44024008	sa so ɔɔ so pɛdarara wɩ ɩna afɩ ƴɛra. Fɩ punone bule kuunikɛra dɩbara a jɩɩ jɩ gɩrɛra dɔnɩ kɩrʋ dɩ sɩ pɩɛraa sor.
44024009	Dɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ ture so pɛrɛɛle aa: Mɛna gɩ ha.
44024010	Dɩ gobanɛr 'laa Polla nyɔ̃ɔ a mɩa, dɩ Pol sʋʋraa: Mɩ jɩrɛ dɩ fɛr dʋɔn so kɩɩldaar ga caraakɛ yɛna jɔɔ; gɛr gɩ mɩ hananɛ 'lar a na mɩɩna ɩ̃ so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ thɩmɩɩ afɩ ƴɛra.
44024011	Jaalɩkɛ mɩ kɔɔ jalnɩ Jerujalɛm a fʋɔr Thãgba, ga ka wire yʋɔr yenyɔa', fɩ punone a jɩ gɩ.
44024012	Sɩ wa kɔɔ yɩ mɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna dɩ ma-n bana thɩ̃ banaa na tibilə', dɩ wa yɩ mɩ wo dɩ ɩ̃ bɛɛ tibil jɔ Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔnanɔ, dɩ le dɩɩra ga.
44024013	Gɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɩrʋ wɩ pɛ marnɩ sor gɩrɛ, wa puno na ti kɩrʋ kpɩɩrakɛ a na nɩna fa'.
44024014	Ma mʋ̃ fara', asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ Thãgba mɩ-n fʋɔr, dɩ ma-n kpana Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ sõso hʋɛ, a pɛrna haar gɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ kherenenɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋra na Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ sɛbɛra.
44024015	Dɩ mɩ hananɛ nũ pɛrɛ Thãgbara mɔ̃kɛ wɛr thɛthɛ hana gɩnɩ wer, dɩ tɩɩ sara na wɩrɛ na sarana' na ɩɩrɛ na the khirera.
44024016	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ma-n do bʋɔ bɔɔ fɛʋ, dɩ ma-n hana kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ na heene mɩnɩ sor Thãgbaa ƴɛra dɩ tɩbɩlala ga.
44024017	Yɛna jɔɔ kɔɔ kar sɩ ma kɔɔ jal Jerujalɛma', sɩ bubul mũsumo mɩ gba jalna a ha ɩ̃ too sa ji bonɩɛ Thãgbara.
44024018	Dɩ thale wɩ yɩ mɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ phʋɔlnɩ pɩ, sɩ ga do tɩɩ jɔ wɩ kɔɔ yɩna ma', dɩ khʋ̃ɛ na kɔɔ hale dakha woa'.
44024019	Ɩkha Juifisɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Ajɩ, wɛr teana wɩ jɩlɛ afɩ ƴɛra a pɛ mar sor, ado wɩ hana mɛr sor.
44024020	A mɛ̃ gaa, wɛr n sɔ dɩbara gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ yɩnɩ dɩɩ do dɩ paar, ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ jɩɩlnɩ so gʋʋrdaraa ƴɛra,
44024021	saagado huleneekɛ dɩbara mɩ kɔɔ huleni awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn ayɩ, khi ɩɩrɛ dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ wa-n kɩɩlna mɩ afɩ ƴɛra gɩrɛ nĩ gaaga.
44024022	Dɩ gɩdonɩ Felɩsɩ jɩɛ jɩ bɔɔbɔɔ mɔ̃ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra n mɩɩnɩ, a so warɛ wɩ tɔɔ, a Lɩjɩasɩ sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋ ɩ̃ gɛr ɩna gʋʋrɔ awɩ so.
44024023	Dɩ a sor sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩna a na-n hɩnɛ Pol sɩ a hanaa hʋɛ, dɩ a na-n pɩɛr dakha ɔɔ too wa-n pɔ a na buluu na thɩ̃aa ga.
44024024	A wire gbe kɔɔ ka, Felɩsɩ pɔr nakha ɔɔ khɛr Durusilikɛ dɔnɩ Juifi, a thɔ̃ a we Pol dɩ pɔ a mɩɩ ha pɛrɛɛkɛ tibil na hananɩ Jeju Kirisitira, dɩ wɩ pɛ nũu.
44024025	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Pol n mɩɩnɩ fɩl sardaa, na dɩbara fʋdaa, na Thãgbaa kɩɩlɩkɛ na ɩnanɩ, maar fʋrɛ Felɩsɩ dɩ so aa: Kɔna mɛ̃ nɛnɛ̃; a mɩ yɩ hʋɛ, ma bire na we fɩ.
44024026	A-n kpɩɛrɛra Pol na ha nɛr war, gɛr gɩ dɩ thɔ̃ tɔ̃tɔ̃tɔ̃ dɩ wɩɩ dɩ wa-n khʋɛ kha.
44024027	Sɩ a yɛna yenyɔ ka pɩ, Pɔrsiyusi Fɛsɩtusi kɔɔ deere Felɩsɩ. Sɩ gɩdonɩ Felɩsɩ ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n da Juifisɔ haar, gɛr gɩ dɩ sɩrɔ Pol le khaɩra.
44025001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Fɛsɩtusi danɩ le, balãther a cɔ sa the le Sejare a jal Jerujalɛm.
44025002	Dɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ na Juifi kɔ̃tɩna gbaar Polɩda a mɩgʋʋ sa phʋʋr Fɛsɩtusi,
44025003	a jɛ wɩ bʋɔra sa cʋɛ Pol a pɔ Jerujalɛm; sɩ jaa wɩ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ sa nʋɔ hʋɛra wɩ kʋʋ.
44025004	Sɩ Fɛsɩtusi birse, Pol hale khaɩra Sejare, dɩ ɩnɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na birə na jal dɔdɔ.
44025005	Dɔ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩna anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn n jal kha na mɛrɛ, dɩ ado dɩkhaa thɩ̃ puu kuunile cʋʋ, nɩ pɩɛraa sor.
44025006	Sɩ Fɛsɩtusi toore Jerujalɛm wire makõther wire yʋɔrsɔ dɩbara, sa gba jal Sejare. Dɩ dɩɩ wɩl dɩ too ɔɔ kɩɩl too pa sa yɩ, wɩ kpa Pol a pɔna.
44025007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a danɩ, Juifisɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Jerujalɛm diirəəre dɩ wa-n pɩɛraa sɔ bərəəm dɩɩ puuro ka. Sɩ ga do wɩ-n marɛ wo dɩ wɩ jɩɩ mɩɩ dɩ sobɔr n yɩra'.
44025008	Dɩ Pol fʋrɛ ɔɔ so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ thɩmɩɩ ayɩ: Ma dɩ Juifisɔɔ jɔfʋra ga, dɩ ma dɩ dakha Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna ga, dɩ Sejaar fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩɩna gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ da'.
44025009	Dɩ Fɛsɩtusiikɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ a da Juifisɔ haar birsere Pol: Fa ture na jal Jerujalɛm dɩ wa kɩɩlna fɩ le ɩ̃ ƴɛra ya?
44025010	Dɩ Pol birsee: Mɩ jɩɩlɛ Sejaarɩ kɩɩl pa, le gɩ teena wɩ kɩɩlna mɩ. Ma dɩ Juifisɔra thɩ̃ bɩɛlla ga, fɛrɛ yɛrɛrakɛ fɩ jɩ gɛr bɔɔbɔɔbɔɔ.
44025011	Ado mɩ cʋʋrɛ dɩkhaa puu, dɩ a dɩkhaa sopugo gɩɩkɛ teananɩ khir ma bo na yɩ ma khəə ga; sɩ ado sorɩkɛra wɩ-n pɛ marnɩ na do sobɔra', tibil na hana hʋɛ a na fʋ mɩ na ha wa'; foo thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ n dã Sejaarɩ pa.
44025012	Le Fɛsɩtusi gʋʋr kha na so gʋʋrdara sa so: Sejaarɩ iikɛ fɩ wenɩ, Sejaarɩ pa fa jal.
44025013	A wire gbe kɔɔ ka, Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar na Berenɩsɩ pɔr le Sejare wɩ fʋɔr Fɛsɩtusi.
44025014	Sɩ mɔ̃ wɩ toonɩ le a na pʋɔr gbe, Fɛsɩtusi gbaar Polɩda a mɩɛ fãgadaarra a so aa: Kũu bɩɛl hakɛ Felɩsɩ faanɩ khaɩra.
44025015	Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ Jerujalɛm, bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnasɔ nakha Juifi kɔ̃tɩnasɔ kɔɔ pɩɛraarɛ sor sa bɩɛl mɩ ɩ̃ heenee sor.
44025016	Sɩ mɩ kɔɔ so warɛ Rɔmɛ̃sɔ na mɩlna tibil gba 'laarɛ, sɩɩ do wa haa hʋɛ dɩ jɩɩl wɩrɛ n pɩɛraanɩ sorɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn na so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛɛkɛ a na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɩ gɩrɛraakɛra wɩ pɩɛraanɩ sor ɓoaa ga.
44025017	Dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ ɩ̃ kha na mɛrɛ; ma kɔɔ pʋɔra', sɩ ga dɩ wɩlla mɩ kɔɔ toore kɩɩl paar sa yɩ wɩ kpa kuunilera a ɛna.
44025018	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩrɛɛkɛra n pɩɛraanɩ sor kɔɔ pɔnɩ, wa kɔɔ pɩɛraa ga so puu caakɛ mɩ kɔɔ pɛrnɩ haar gɛr wa pɩɛraa ga.
44025019	Sɩ wɩ kɔɔ hananɛ sor dɩɩ do awɩ Thãgba fʋɔrda gɩ-n hɩɩn dɩbara dɔrɔɔm, na tibil bɩɛllaakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jejuukɛ kɔɔ khenɩ, sɩ dɩ Polla n so dɩ yɩ aa: Gel, a hananɛ yire.
44025020	Dɩ gɩdonɩ ma jɩɩ jɩ mɔ̃ ma 'lonɩ ga so caala', mɩ kɔɔ bulele Pol ado a na ture na jal Jerujalɛm dɩ wa kɩɩlnaa le ga soolera.
44025021	Sɩ gɩdonɩ Pol wer Sejaarɩ i, a ƴaal wɩ sɛ nar ɔr fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ n gʋʋr ɩnɩ so, dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so wa-n bɛraa phaphapha ɩ̃ thɔnaa Sejaarɩ para.
44025022	Dɩ Agɩrɩpa so Fɛsɩtusira: Mɛrɛ dakha, mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ pɛ kuunilee thɩmɩɩra nũu. Dɩ Fɛsɩtusi birsee: Cʋɔ fa nɩɛrɛ ɔɔ nɔ.
44025023	Gɛr gɩ dɩ dɩɩ wɩl dɩ Agɩrɩpa na Berenɩsɩ pɔ dakpɛ pʋɔ, a lõ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩ cʋɔrɔ na sɔrasɛɛ sɛfʋsɔ na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ dɩɩra. Dɩ Fɛsɩtusi so wɩ kpa Pol a pɔna.
44025024	Le Fɛsɩtusi so aa: Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar, na nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩkɛ gɩrɛ na sɛrɛ, nɩ yɩrɛ kuunikɛ Juifisɔ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ Jerujalɛm na kɛkɛdara bɩɛl mɩnɩ dɩ wa-n hulena: Ga teena a hana yire bã.
44025025	Ado mɛrra gɩ, mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ do aa cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ teananɩ khirə', sɩ gɩdonɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛ wɛ Sejaarɩ i, mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ bɔr dɩ a na jal le.
44025026	Ma jɩɩ jɩ bɔɔbɔɔ gɩrɛɛkɛ ma kherenɩ ɔɔdarara a na ha fãgadaar kɔ̃tɩ̃a'. Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ɩ̃ kpaa ɩna anɩ ƴɛra, sɩ caca afɩ ƴɛra, fɛr Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar, dɩ mɛ̃ ma jɩ gɩrɛ ma kherenɩ ado fɩ gʋʋr ɔɔda a hɩɩn.
44025027	Gɩdonɩ, ado mɛrra gɩ, ga tee kha a mɩ thɔna Sejaarra khaɩdaar sɩ ma so sorɩkɛ wɩ pɩɛraanaa ga.
44026001	Dɩ Agɩrɩpa so Polla: Wɩ ha fɛr hʋɛ dɩ fa mɩɩ afɩ so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ ɩhɩmɩɩ. Dɩ Pol 'laa nyɔ̃ɔ da-n mɩɩ ɔɔ so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ thɩmɩɩ thaa ayɩ:
44026002	Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar, mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ do ɩ̃ nɔbɔ gɩ dɩ ma-n kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ na hɛl afɩ ƴɛra nĩ ɩ̃ so fɛʋʋkɛra Juifisɔ pɛ marnɩ gɩrɛ,
44026003	gɩdonɩ fɩ jɩɛ jɩ bɔɔbɔɔbɔɔ Juifisɔɔ mama fɩl fɛʋ na awɩ thɩ̃ banasɔ; gɛr gɩ mɩ-n bɩɛl fɛr dɩ fa pɛ mɩ nũu na ha fʋrɛ.
44026004	A fʋna caca fʋ paar ɩ̃ daɓol dĩi bɔɔ, Juifisɔ fɛʋ jɩrɛ mɔ̃ ɩ̃ fɩl hanɩ gɩdonɩ Jerũjalɛm mɩ kɔɔ ha ɩ̃ caa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
44026005	Wɩ kɔɔ mãa jɩ mar kɛkɛkɛ, ado wɩ-n ƴaalɛ wɩ so sobɔr, dɩ mɛr dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ hananɩ jɔfʋ bʋ dʋ fɩlɛ a ɓã wɛkɛra hanɩ awɩ ƴɛra kpɩɩ, kɛ n jɩɛnnɩ hɩɩn bɔɔbɔɔ asɩ Thãgba fʋɔr fɩl.
44026006	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ wɩ-n kɩɩlna mɛr gɩrɛ, gɩdonɩ mɩ hananɛ nũ pɛrɛ ʋlfɛrɛraakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ,
44026007	ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ asɩ ca ƴʋɔr yenyɔ n yɩrrɔnɩ dɩ wa-n fʋɔr Thãgba dɩtɩnɔ na dɩwɩlʋ, dɩ wa-n pɩɛrna mɔ̃ ʋlfɛrɛɛlera na danɩ na ha oti. Fãgadaar, ga nũ pɛɛlera dɔ kɩrʋ Juifisɔ pɛ marnɩ sor gɩrɛ.
44026008	Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n pɛr haar dɩ Thãgba na cʋʋrɛ khe dɩ wa ɩɩr na the khirera ga?
44026009	Ado mɛrra kɔɔ gɩ, mɩ kɔɔ kpɩɛrɛ sa bãba a cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ gɩ kʋɛara Najarɛtɩ Jejuu i.
44026010	Thale mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋ Jerujalɛm. Mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ khaanɛ tɩɩ phuusɔ jɔɔ khaɩra, gɩdonɩ mɛ̃ mɩ kɔɔ bɩɛl hʋɛ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩnaa pa; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ yɩnɩ wɩ kʋrɛ wɩ, mɩ kɔɔ ture ayɩ: Gɩ hana mɛ̃.
44026011	Mɩ-n kɔɔ heen wer sor Juifisɔɔ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔra bɔɔ fɛʋ, dɩ ma-n yɩrna wɩ wɩ kʋɛa Jejuu i. Sɩ gɩdonɩ nɩ̃khii thʋnɛ ka mɩ, mɩ-n kɔɔ kpoo warɛ na wɩrɛ hanɩ bə̃ kpɩɩrarakɛ.
44026012	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ mɩ-n kɔɔ jaalnɩ Damasɩ, gɩdonɩ bonɩ jidaar kɔ̃tɩna kɔɔ ha mɛr hʋɛ.
44026013	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ mɩ hanɩ hʋɛra, fãgadaar, ʋlkhɔɔ gɩ kɔɔ do, dɩ dahɩrɛ kɔɔ ther ƴũ a thʋ̃ carã a jɔ wi hɩrɛrɛ, a dii mar na wɩrɛ sɩ-n kɔɔ jalnanɩ kha.
44026014	Dɩ sɩ jiir fɛʋ thʋnɔ sɩ dɩ ɩ̃ nɩɛ wire dɩɩ so mar na ebirə thɩmɩɩr ayɩ: Sɔl, Sɔl, mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ fa-n kpoo mar mɛna? Dɩbara fɩ-n cʋʋ puure mɔ̃ na na-n banɩ na gɔdaa na nɔɔ.
44026015	Dɩ ɩ̃ birsee: Kɔ̃tɩn, fɛr amɛ gɩ? Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn so: Mɛr dʋɔn Jejuukɛ fɩ-n kpooronɩ.
44026016	Sɩ ɩrɛ jɩlɛ. Mɛr gbaan dɩbara a nɩna fɩ. Mɩ thɩɩn fɛr fɩ do ɩ̃ thɔ̃daar na ɩ̃ sobɔ so jɩdaar gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ yɩnɩ mɛrɛra, na gɩrɛraakɛra fa yɩnɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ma birni na gba dɩbara a na nɩna fɩ wo.
44026017	Dɩ ma taa fɛr tɩbɩlaakɛɛ nyɔ̃kɔɔ na ca kpalaa nyɔ̃kɔɔ kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ ma thɔ̃ farnɩ,
44026018	fɩ khɛr wɩ yinə, wɩ the dabirəra wɩ lõ dahɩrɛra, wɩ the Satãa fãgara wɩ kɛr wɩ pɛ Thãgba haar, wɩ 'lɛ sopugo faarɛ na awɩdaakɛ wa hɩnɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgba leenɩ kpɩɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn ha pɛrɛraakɛ wa hananɩ mɛrɛra.
44026019	Dɩ gɛr gɩ, Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar, ma kɔɔ nʋʋr nũu thɩ̃ yɩrraale thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa ga.
44026020	Sɩ Damasɩdara mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ ɓo, agɩpɩ dɩ ɩ̃ mɩɩ Jerujalɛmdara na Judedara fɛʋ nakha ca kpala, wɩ deba haar sa kɛra na kpa Thãgbara, a cʋɛ dakha thɔmaakɛ na nɛnanɩ dɩ wɩ debire haar.
44026021	Gelela dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ fʋ mɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩnɔ a yɩrna mɩna wɩ kʋ.
44026022	Sɩ Thãgba taa mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ hana yire a dana nĩkɛ, dɩ ma-n mɩɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ tɩɩ mɔlɔsɔra na tɩɩ kɔ̃tɩnana, sɩ ma-n golõ thɩ̃ bɩɛllaakɛrakɛ Thãgbaa bobona na Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sonɩ ayɩ ga daana';
44026023	gɛr dɔ mɔ̃ Kirisiti na gaarnɩ bʋɔ sɩ na do cacadaarɩkɛ na kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ na the khirera a na mɩɩ dahɩrɛɛda Juifisɔra na ca kpalala.
44026024	Mɔ̃kɛ Pol n mɩɩnɩ ɔɔ so hɛl kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ thɩmɩɩ thakɛ, Fɛsɩtusi sor na nɔ kheu aa: Pol, yʋʋ kʋɛa fɩ, afɩ jɩ jɔjɔra kʋɛa fɩ yʋʋ.
44026025	Dɩ Pol birsee: Fɛr, Fɛsɩtusi bʋɔ, yʋʋ na kʋɛ ma', sobɔ thɩmɩɩr na yʋ bɔ thɩmɩɩr mɩ ka ma-n mɩɩ.
44026026	Mɩ mɩɩrɛ Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar na 'lar gɩdonɩ a jɩrɛ ga thɩ̃sɔɔle; gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩrɛ dɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛl na hale aa jɩnaa ga, gɩdonɩ ga do gelela kɔɔ wolone dã ga.
44026027	Fɩ pɛrɛ Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ thɩmɩɩ haar ya, Agɩrɩpa fãgadaar? Mɩ jɩrɛ fɩ pɛrɛ haar.
44026028	Dɩ Agɩrɩpa so Polla: Gɩ do fɩ yɩrna mɛr bɔɔ gberaakɛ dɩ ɩ̃ do Kirisitiida bɛɛ?
44026029	Dɩ Pol birsee: A nɛnɛ̃ gɩ, a dɩkhõo gɩ yoo, mɩ-n bɩɛlɛ Thãgba dɩ ga-n do fɛrɛ dɩbara ga, sɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n pɛ mɩnɩ nũu nĩ n deba a hana mɔ mɩ hanɩ, sɩ jɔrkɔ lir na-n hala'.
44026030	Dɩ fãgadaar, na gobanɛr, na Berenɩsɩ, na wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ tɔɔna wɩnɩ ɩɩr
44026031	a thɩɩr dɩ wa-n mɩɩ khasɔ aa: Sa yɩ kuunnaakɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ teena khir agɩbo khaɩ pɛra'.
44026032	Dɩ Agɩrɩpa so Fɛsɩtusira: Wɩ kɔɔ punone faa kuunikɛ adora aa kɔɔ we Sejaarɩ iə'.
44027001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ gʋʋrnɩ sa yɩ sɩ lona bato a jala Ɩtalɩ, wɩ gbaar Pol na wɩ̃ khaɩdara a pɛ Juliyusii nyɔ̃kɔɔ; ɔr dɔ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ Ogusitii sɔrasɩsɔra.
44027002	Sɩ kɔɔ gbaar batookɛ thɛnɩ Adɩramɩtɩ da-n jal dɩɩraakɛ hanɩ Ajɩ lanyɔ̃ gẽgerena; dɩ mɛ̃ sɩ lõ jal, sɩ Arɩsɩtarkɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Masedʋandaar, kɛ thɛnɩ Tesalonɩkɩ sɩ kɔɔ hana kha.
44027003	Dɩ dɩɩ na wɩl dɩɩ do sɩ daan Sɩdɔ̃. Juliyusiikɛ n hɩnɛnɩ Pol na fɩl bʋɔ kɔɔ haarɛ hʋɛ dɩ jal ɔɔ kuunsɔɔ pa wɩ buluu.
44027004	Dɩ sɩ the le a gba bato a kana Sɩpɩr yɔ dɩ gɛlʋ, gɩdonɩ jɩɛ thʋnɛ telẽ sɩ ka.
44027005	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ lanyʋɔnɩkɛ n celanɩ da-n pɛ Silisi na Pãfɩlɩ dɩɩra, sɩ kɔɔ daan Mɩraakɛ dɔnɩ Lisi dɩ bɩɛl.
44027006	Le sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ yɩ batookɛ thɛnɩ Alesãdɩɩrɩ da-n jal Ɩtalɩ dɩ sɩ lõ.
44027007	Sɩ kɔɔ jaal hɛlɛlɛ a cʋʋna wire jɔɔ; gɩ khɩɩ sarɛ ka dɩ sa lõ Kiniidi, gɩdonɩ jɩɛ na ha sɩ jalʋa'. Sɩ kɔɔ kananɛ tɩɛr Kɩrɛtɩ yɔ dɩɩ Salmɔn khʋra.
44027008	Mɛna gɩ khe sar dɩ sɩ fʋ gẽgerẽ nʋɔ phaphapha a jal dã paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Bopɔɔr, ka Laje dɩɩ wɔrɔnɩ.
44027009	Bɔ jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ kar sɩ dɩ jaal debi a puuro ka, gɩdonɩ bɔɔkɛ sopugo hɛl bonɩ ji bɔɔ kɔɔ kanɩ gɩ do. Gɛr gɩ dɩ Pol kpãkpãa war ayɩ:
44027010	Kona, mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩ asɩ jalla na nɩ sɛr na ka, dɩ ga dor thɩ̃ kʋɛrɛ na ka; ga do bato gɩ na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hanɩle bɩnɔ dɩbara ga, sɩ asɩ thɛthɛrakɛ dakha.
44027011	Sɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ kɔɔ pɛr ʋrɛ n cananɩ bato na bato hɩ̃daarɩ thɩmɩɩ nũu, sa ka bo Polɩda.
44027012	Sɩ gɩdonɩ jɩɩl paarɩle na bɔr dɩ bato na tooro yʋʋrɔa', ɩkhasɔ jɔɔ sor: Sɩ thɛ le a dɔ bʋɔ a dana Fenɩsɩ, Kɩrɛtɩ bato jɩɩl pa ka 'weenenɩ gananɔ, dɩ le sa too yʋʋrɔ.
44027013	Sɩ jɩɛ kɔɔ ther wi phã paar nyɔ̃bɩlana da-n phʋ̃ fɛlɛlɛlɛ, dɩ wɩ ka jɩna ɩnɩ punone dɩbara, a ɩɩr hal bato fʋ ther a ti sɩ dɩɩ fʋ Kɩrɛtɩ yɔ dɩ gẽgerẽ nʋɔ dɩ ga-n jal.
44027014	Ga pʋɔra', sɩ jɛ kʋkʋʋlʋʋkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Erakɩlɔ̃ kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ yɔ dɩɩraale,
44027015	a gba bato dɩ ga-n jalna dɩ ga-n puno dɩɩ telẽ jɩɛ bã, gɛr gɩ dɩ sɩ faa bɔ dʋʋr dɩɩ gba sɩ a jalna.
44027016	Dɩ sɩ kana tɩɛr yɔ dɩ buurəəkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Kʋloda, ka sɩ 'lɛnɩ puɩɩone gbe, mɔ̃ gɩ nɩ sɩnɩ mɛna sɩ sɩ marrɛ bato buu a gba pɛ batora.
44027017	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ khəini bato buu a pɛ batora, wɩ gbaar pɔ̃ɔ a parna bato dɩɩ ma. Gɩdonɩ maar fʋ wɛr dɩ agakpaana wa jaal na ti Sɩrtɩ gbalãkothɩnna, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ ti jɛ kɩ̃kɩɩn. Thale jɩɛ kɔɔ gba wɩ a jalna.
44027018	Mɔ̃kɛ jɛkhureele n bɩɩr sɩnɩ na fãga mɛ̃, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ tiir thɩ̃ɛ ga dɩ wɩlla a dʋʋrna lanyʋɔnɔ;
44027019	dɩ balãther wire, wɛr thɛthɛ gbaan bato thɩ̃ɛ na awɩ nyɛ̃ a dʋʋrna faa.
44027020	Wire na ƴepələ̃be na kɔɔ yɩr wi jɔjʋɔraala'; mɔ̃ jɛkhureele n be sɩnɩ na fãga mɛna sa-n kpɩɛr sa taarɛ 'lo bã.
44027021	Gɩ pʋɔrɛ sɩ tibil na kɔɔ kho dɩkora'. Le Pol ɩɩr awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a jɩɩl a so war ayɩ: Kona, adora nɩ kɔɔ pɛr mɛr nũu ga dor sa kɔɔ the Kɩrɛtɩ yɔ dɩɩra a na yɩ nɩ caakɛ na thɩ̃ kʋɛ caaka'.
44027022	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ mɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr, nɩ pɩɛr 'lar gɩdonɩ tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra na buə', sɩ bato dɩbara na kʋɛa.
44027023	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaakɛ hɩna mɩnɩ dɩ ma-n dʋʋraa thɔma, ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ the marɛ dɩtɩnɔɔkɛ
44027024	a so mar ayɩ: Pol; aa, ma-n do maar n fʋ ma', dɔ ɩ̃ jal ɩ̃ jɩɩl Sejaarɩ ƴɛra aa, sɩ ɩ̃ hɩnɛ, Thãgba ha mɛr wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ batoraakɛ na mɛrɛ.
44027025	Gɛr gɩ kona, nɩ pɩɛr 'lar gɩdonɩ mɩ hananɛ tu jɩɩr Thãgbaa pa dɩ ga har mɔna a so marnɩ.
44027026	Sɩ jɩɛ wer na gba sɛr na jalna yɔ dɩ bɩɛlla.
44027027	Dɩtɩnɛ yʋɔr yenãdaara ɔbɔɔle sɩ-n kpaar bababa Adɩrɩatɩkɩ lanyʋɔnɔ, dɩnɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn batodara ka jɩna sɩ-n wɔrɔnɛ thɩɩ.
44027028	Gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ mɩɛ yɔ hulone a hɩɩn na pɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ linəni ther a yɩɛ dɩɩ thɔɔ mɛtɛrɛ kpalanyɔ; a wɩ jal gbe wo, wɩ bire mɩɛ yɔ hulone a hɩɩn a yɩɛ dɩɩ thɔɔ mɛtɛrɛ kpelẽ yʋɔr.
44027029	Sɩ maar fʋ wɛr agakpaana bato na thʋrɛ bokaar, gɛr gɩ dɩ wɩ dʋna bato fʋ thɛ yenã bato sɩkaar, gɩ fɔ bato gɩ jɩɩl sɩ wa-n jɩ ʋmɔ̃ bɔɔ dɩɩ na wɩlna'.
44027030	Sɩ batodara kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ faa bato sɩ wɩ caalɛ a gba bato buu a kpɛɛ nyʋɔnɔ, sɩ jaa wɩ-n ƴaalɛ wɩ caalɛ sa cʋʋ dɩɩ ho wɩ yɛ, bato fʋ ther ɩnɩ-n kpɛɛ ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ gɩ fɔ bacto.
44027031	Dɩ Pol sor sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩna na sɔrasɛsɔra ayɩ: Ado tibil yɩrɛ na too kɛ bato bɩnɔa', na puno na yɩ taa paara'.
44027032	Le sɔrasɛ kuur pɛ̃ɛkɛ fɔnɩ bato buu a faa dɩɩ ji nyʋɔnɔ.
44027033	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ n thɔɔnɩ wɩllɛ, Pol sor tɩbɩlala fɛʋ ayɩ wɩ khɔ dɩkor; a so warɛ wo: Wire yʋɔr yenã ha gɩrɛ nĩ nɩ toonɩ pɩɛrɔ a bona dɩkor.
44027034	Gɛr gɩ mɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr, nɩ khɔ dɩkor gɩdonɩ gɛr na bulo ni dɩ na taa, gɩdonɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩnɩ yʋsũ na buə'.
44027035	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a mɩɩnɩ thale pɩ, gɛr a gbaar buru a bɩɛl Thãgba a pɛr wɛr fɛʋʋ ƴɛra; agɩpɩ dɩ kur a ma da-n kho.
44027036	Dɩ fɛʋ kɔɔ pɛrɛ 'lar a kho wer oti.
44027037	Sɛrkɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ hanɩ bato bɩnɔɔle, sɩ kɔɔ har taanyɔ na kpalãther yʋɔr maadõ.
44027038	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ khonɩ dɩkor a hi, wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ bato dɩɩ haba, gɩdonɩ wɩ dʋʋrnanɛ bile lanyʋɔnɔ.
44027039	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩɩ wɩlnɩ, wa kɔɔ jɩ bəən bã, sɩ wɩ kɔɔ 'laarɛ yɩ paarɩkɛ nyʋɔn n lonanɩ thɩɩra, kɛ na dɔnɩ dahulõ paara'; dɩ wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n tɔna bato a jalana le ado ɩna punone.
44027040	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ thʋbɩrɛ bato fʋ thɛ a faa dɩɩ jal lanyʋɔnɔ, dɩ wɩ thʋbɩrɛ pɛ̃ɛkɛ wɩ kɔɔ gbanɩ a linə bato thɔɔdaasɔ, sa khəi ƴɛbʋ kɩ̃kɩɩn a pɛr jɩɛ batora gɩ gba bato gɩ jalna gɩ dana gẽgerẽ nʋɔra.
44027041	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ danɩ kãkɛ lanyʋɔn n caannɩ dɩ a-n be kha, bato kɔɔ thʋnɔnɛ sa gɔ gbalãkothɩnna dɩ mɩ̃kaar mar kĩkĩkĩ ga-n tutugə'; sɩ sɩkaar ma dɩ a-n kʋɛ, nyʋɔn n cɩr gɩnɩ mɛna.
44027042	Dɩ sɔrasɛsɔ ƴaalɛ wɩ kʋʋr khaɩdara, gɩdonɩ wɩ kpɩɛrɛ ʋkha na pher na fuu.
44027043	Sɩ sɔrasɛ tamaa kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ ƴaalɛnɩ a taa Pol a pɩɛr wɛr wa-n cʋa'. Dɩ a so warɛ ayɩ: Wɩrɛ jɛnɩ phɩɩr, wɛr n kɔɔ je nyʋɔnɔ caca a phɛ thɛ;
