44027044	sɩ wɩrɛ sɛnɩ n fɔ thɩra, agɩbo wɩ fʋ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hanɩ batora wa-n phe; mɛ̃ wɛr fɛʋ dã thɩɩ pɔlpɔlpɔl.
44028001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ taanɩ pɩ, gɛr sɩ jɩrɔ dɩɩ do yɔ dɩɩlera wɩ-n we Maltɩ.
44028002	Dɩdaraale kɔɔ dona sɛr bʋɔ ka; wɩ kɔɔ kpa sɛr fɛʋ dɩ sɩ ɩɩr dɔ jɔjʋɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ gbɔɔnɩ, gɩdonɩ thãgba n daan dɩ ɩɩr thʋ̃ kar.
44028003	Dɩ Pol kɔɔ paalɛ sɔ̃sʋɔnɛ a pɛ dɔɔ, dɩ dɔ kporre tire dɔ̃phaanʋ dɩ the a maa nyɔ̃ɔ.
44028004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ dɩdaraale yɩnɩ siile dɩ juu nyɔɔna, wɩ-n mɩɩrɛ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl aa: Sobɔr gɩ, kuunikɛ tɩɩ kʋ gɩ, a taarɛ lanyʋɔnna wer pɩ, sɩ thãgbaakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ dasarʋ na sɩɩraa da la'.
44028005	Sɩ Pol jɛbɩrɛ siile dɔɔra sɩ aa kɔɔ nɩ khoo fɩɩʋraka'.
44028006	Dɩ tɩbɩlaale n pɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ ga bʋnɩna, agɩbo mɔ̃ a na təəni na ji na khi dapaara; sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ pɩɛrnɩ ƴɛrr sɩ wa yɩ thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ puurəə ga, wɩ debire kpɩɛrɛ wo a so aa: Dɩ thãgba haarakaa ya?
44028007	Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl hale ga yɔ dɩraalera dɩ wa-n wɩɩ Pubiliyusi a hana lɩɛ; ɔr tea sɩ na fɩl bʋɔ dɩ sɩ too ɔɔ cɔ wire yẽther;
44028008	sɩ khoo kɔɔ fʋrɛ Pubiliyusii thɩ, tomɩ kporre gɩ na khʋɔnɛ. Dɩ Pol lõ a yɩɩ a dɛɛnaa nyɛ̃ɛ sa bɩɛl Thãgba a pɩɛraa dɩ kpɛɛ.
44028009	A gele ka pɩ, wɩ̃ khodaarsɔɔkɛ hanɩ yɔ dɩɩraale pɔr a kpɛɛ awɩ khosɔ.
44028010	Wɩ-n cʋ sɛr dɩɩ pho ka, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ-n thenɩ le wɩ kɔɔ ha sɛr gɩrɛɛkɛ n ɓɔra sɩnɩ.
44028011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ toonɩ le dɩ pora yẽther ka, sɩ lʋʋn batookɛ wɩ-n wenɩ thãgba bi ƴɔna, kɛ thɛnɩ Alesãdɩɩrɩ, kɛ kɔɔ tɔɔnɩ le yɔ dɩɩraale yʋʋrɔ.
44028012	Mɔ̃ sɩ danɩ Sɩrakusi, sɩ kɔɔ toore le wire yẽther.
44028013	Dɩ le sɩ kɔɔ jalna gẽgerẽ nʋɔ a dã Rejiyo. A ga dɩ wɩl, jɩɛ kɔɔ ther wi phã paar nyɔ̃bɩlana a gba sɩ, dɩ ga cʋʋ wire yenyɔ dɩɩ do sɩ daan dapaara Pujɔl,
44028014	kãkɛ sɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ omɩna, dɩ wɩ bɩɛl sɩ sɩ tɔɔ le a cʋɛ wire makonyɔ. Thale sɩ kɔɔ dã Rɔm.
44028015	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ omɩna nɩɛnɩ dɩ sɩ har hʋɛra, wɩ kɔɔ caan sɛr paarsɔɔkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Apiyusi ƴatɛ na Kpakpal cɔna yẽther; dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Pol hanɩ na yɩ wɩ a pɛrɛ 'lar sa khɩɩ Thãgba.
44028016	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ danɩ Rɔm, wɩ har Pol hʋɛ a na-n cɔ dɩbara na sɔrasɩ bɩɛlɩkɛ n hɩnɛɛnɩ.
44028017	A wire yẽther ka, Pol wer Juifi kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ gbɛbɩnɩ kha a so warɛ thɩmɩaakɛ ayɩwɔɔ: Omɩna, ma kɔɔ cʋʋ tɩbɩla puurə', dɩ ma dɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ fɩlla woa', sɩ wɩ kɔɔ fʋ mɛr a to khaɩra Jerujalɛm sa gba mɩ ha Rɔmɛ̃sɔ.
44028018	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ bule mini thɩ̃ɛ pɩ, wɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛla wɩ faa mɩ gɩdonɩ wa yɩ mar thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ teananɩ khirə'.
44028019	Sɩ Juifisɔ n kɔɔ yɩrna mɛr dɩ ɩ̃ tha thʋnɔ sa yɩ: Foo dɩ thɩmɩɩrra Sejaarɩ pa ga dã, sɩrakɛ ga do sor mɩ hana dɩ ma-n pɛ ɩ̃ cara ga.
44028020	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ɩ̃ we nɩ ɩ̃ mɩɛ nɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ, gɩdonɩ Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsanaa nũ pɛ dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ wɩ li mi na jɔrkɔɔkɛ.
44028021	Dɩ wɩ birsee: Sa kɔɔ 'lɛ sɛbɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ Jude dɩɩra afɩ sora ga, dɩ omine gɩ a gba fɩ ɩna kɛ a mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ puu a pɛ fara'.
44028022	Sɩ sɩ-n ƴaalɛ sɩ nɩ afɩ nɔ sɩ jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ fɩ-n kpɩɛrnɩ, gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ paar fɛʋ tɩbɩla n kɛ̃kɛrɛnanɛ dɩɩr caakɛra hanɩ kpɩɩ.
44028023	Dɩ wɩ dʋrɛ wire dɩ tɩbɩla jɔɔ pɔ ka a-n cɔnɩ a ƴɩɩ. Dɩ Pol mɩɩ wɛr Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda dɩ wɩ hɩɩn, a mɩɩna wɛr sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩr a gbana Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ na Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔda dɩ yɩrna da-n mɩɛ wɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Jejuuda. Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ toore kha duuro a dana dʋɔrɔ.
44028024	Dɩ ɩkhasɔ n ture gɩrɛɛkɛ a sonɩ, sɩ ɩkhasɔ na-n tuə'.
44028025	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ nʋɔ na-n mãkha wɩnɩ kha ga dɩ wa-n bɩlã, Pol so warɛ thakɛ dɩbara ayɩ: Gɩrɛɛkɛra Thu Phuu kɔɔ gbanɩ Ejaɩ Thãgbaa bobonɩ nɔ a mɩɩna anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, dor sobɔr waa gel ayɩ:
44028026	“Jala tɩbɩlaakɛɛ pa a sɔ war ayɛ: Na-n nɩɛrɛ na anɩ nũ wer bɔɔbɔɔ, sɩ na jɩ kɩrʋa'; na-n hɩɩnɛ na anɩ yi wer bɔɔbɔɔ, sɩ na yɩ ga.
44028027	Gɩdonɩ tɩbɩlaakɛɛ ha dibire; wɩ sɔbɩrɛ awɩ nũ ka, a khaan dakha awɩ yi, a mɛ̃ gaa, ga hor wa yɩ gɛr na awɩ yi, a na nɩɛna awɩ nũ, a na jɩna kɩrʋ, a na kɛr na bir mar dɩ mɛr Thãgba na kpɛɛ wɩ.”
44028028	Gɛr gɩ nɩ jɛna, dɩ Thãgbaa taakɛ ca kpalala a thɔna, dɩ wɛr na pɩɛn nũu.
44028029	[Ɔbɔɔkɛ a sonɩ gele, Juifisɔ n kʋɔn na thɩ̃ banaa jɔjʋɔ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.]
44028030	Sɩ Pol toore yɛna yenyɔ biləni cʋɔrraakɛ a-n lɩmɩnɩ; a-n teere wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n pʋɔnnɩ dɩ wa-n yɩɩ,
44028031	da-n mɩɩna war Thãgbaa fãgadaar doda, da-n dɩɩrna gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩnɩda na 'lar, sɩ tibil na-n pɩɛrʋa'.
45001001	Mɛr Polɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃daar thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ; Thãgba kɔɔ wɛ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ do thɔ̃thɔn, dɩ thɩɩn mɩ kpɩɩ ma-n mɩa tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara.
45001002	Tutugo bʋɔɔkɛra dɔ gɩrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ maanɩ ʋlfɛrɛ dɩ ɩna thɔnanɛ, dɩ ɔɔ bobonasɔ kɔɔ gba a pɛr ɔɔ sɛbɛ phurə.
45001003	Dɩ ɔɔ Bikuunida gɩ mɩɩ; ado kʋɔnnaakɛ tibil kʋɔnɩ gɩ, gɛr a dʋʋr Davɩdɩɩ məl,
45001004	sɩ ado Thãgba dʋʋrra gɩ, na mɔ̃ a donɩ ʋrɛ phonɩ, khireraakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ɩɩrʋʋnɩ na fãga gɛr nɛna dɩ Thãgbaa Bikuun a do.
45001005	Jeju Kirisitiilera dɔnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃, ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ Thãgba jɩ sɩ bʋɔra dɩ sɩ doro gɩrɛ thɔ̃thɔna, gɩ do nɔɔ sɩ gba ɔɔ i sɩ kpana tibil caar fɛʋ sɩ ɩna wɩ pɛr haar wa-n nɩ nũu.
45001006	Dɩ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ harrɛ ner, nɛrɛɛkɛ Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ wenɩ dɩ nɩ do ɔɔda.
45001007	Mɛr Pol thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ hanɩ Rɔm dɩɩra, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ Thãgba n nanɩ a we wɩ dɩ wɩ do tibil phuusɔ. Thãgba asɩ Thɩ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn n hana nɩ ha ɩɩ, a jɛ nɩ dakha bʋɔra.
45001008	Caca thɩ̃ɛ ɩ̃ Thãgba mɩ-n khɩɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋʋ sora dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the, gɩrɛraakɛ wɩ-n mɩɩnɩ anɩ ha pɛda thɩɩraakɛ koo.
45001009	Thãgbaakɛ mɩ-n doronɩ thɔma na haar fɛʋ, ɔɔ Bikuuni tutugo bɔ thɩmɩɩra, torre yire mɔ̃ mɩ-n jɩna nɩnɩ
45001010	ɩ̃ Thãgba bɩɛlla wire fɛʋ, dɩ ma-n phʋʋrʋʋ ado a na ture na ha mɩ hʋɛ ɩ̃ pɔ dɩphãakɛ ɩ̃ yɩ nɩ.
45001011	Gɩdonɩ mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ka ɩ̃ yɩ nɩ, ɩ̃ ha nɩ dɩkhaa Thu Phuu khaarda nɩ 'lɛ fãga;
45001012	kɩrʋ dʋɔn gɩ do bul kha gɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ma hanɩ anɩ pa, anɩ ha pɛ n ha mɩ 'lar, ɩ̃da n ha nɩ 'lar oti.
45001013	Omɩna, ma-n ƴaal na-n jɩ mɔ̃ gɩrɛ hanaa ga; nɩ jɛ dɩ mɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ ƴaalƴaal ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa, sɩ thɩ̃ɛ kɔɔ pɩɛr mɛr a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ dɩ ma kɔɔ yɩ hʋɛa'. Gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ dʋɔn ɩ̃ yɛ tɩbɩla wɩ pɛr Kirisiti haar anɩ pa, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ hanɩ ca kpɩɩsɔɔ pa.
45001014	Mɩ hananɛ wɩrɛ phuoni yire na wɩrɛ na phuoni yirə' helu, na wɩrɛ jɛnɩ sɛbɛ na wɩrɛ na jɛnɩ sɛba' dakha.
45001015	Gɛr gɩ mɩ-n ƴaalɛ na sobɔr ɩ̃ mɩɩ nɩ dakha tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ nɛrɛɛkɛ hanɩ Rɔm.
45001016	Gɩdonɩ yicuru na-n fʋ mι tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmɩɩra ga, Thãgbaa fãga gɩ a do taadaa tibil wo tibilləəkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar, dɩ Juifisɔ wɛ cacaca agɩpɩ wɩrɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa'.
45001017	Gɩdonɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ n nɛna mɔ̃ Thãgba na cʋʋnι dι sor na hɛl tιbιlala ɔɔ ƴɛra, dι ha pɛrɛra gι the fʋ paar a dana pιpιι paar, a ha mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonι ayι: “Ʋrɛ Thãgba hɛllɔnι sor dιι do ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ, ɔr na hana yire.”
45001018	Thãgba n nιnanɛ mɔ̃ a ιιrnanι nĩkhii le ƴũ dιι gbũ a heen Thagba so beesire, na puu cʋʋrɛɛkɛ tιbιla hananι a pιɛrna sobɔr ga-n yιra'.
45001019	Gιdonι gιrɛ tibil na jιnanι Thãgba gι yιr warɛ casι; Thãgba kɔɔ cʋɛ wι wι jɛ gι.
45001020	A fʋna bɔɔkɛ Thãgba tini thɩ̃ɛ, ɔɔ khorr fãga na ɔɔ Thãgba dookɛ na dɔnι dayιnana', gι yιrrɛ casι dι tibil na puno na yι gι, dι gι ther thιɛnaakɛ a tini, dι ga hana tibil n puno a yιrɔ phʋɔl paara'.
45001021	Mɔ̃ wι jιnιnakɛ Thãgba sι wa-n dʋbʋʋ mɔ̃ a donι Thãgba ga, dι wo wa-n fʋɔrʋa', sι awι kpιɛrnɔ debire a do mɔlɔ kpιɛrɛ, dι awι haakɛ dɔnι də̃bəəl haar gι birə warɛ.
45001022	Sι wι-n mιιrɛ mɔ̃ wa donι fιl jιna kpãkpalã ga, sιι do də̃bəəl yire wι debi do.
45001023	Thãgbaakɛ hιnanι i dʋbιrɛ, kɛ na dɔnι dakhinənəə fʋɔr wι ka bo, sι wa-n fʋɔr thιlaakɛ wι cʋʋnι dιι ho tibilikɛ dɔnι dakhinəne, dι wa-n fʋɔrna thιlaakɛ wι-n cʋʋnι dιι ho 'lominə, na nɛɛ yenã thɩ̃ɛ, na thɩ̃ ƴιrɛ n puuloneni.
45001024	Gɛrra dɔ kιrʋ dι Thãgba sι war le awι thɩ̃ bise cʋʋraakɛ n kɔ wιnι thue, dι mɛ̃ wι-n ƴɔ̃ƴɔ̃ɔ awι thɛthɛɛ tomι dιbara ʋ na ʋ.
45001025	Wɛr dɔ wιrɛ fenι Thãgbaa sobɔ dιι do sõsor, sι dι wι fʋɔr a na cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛ thɩ̃ tinənena sa ka faa thɩ̃ Tidaar, kɛ teananι khιιrɛ waa khorr. Amɛn.
45001026	Gɛrra dɔ kιrʋ dι Thãgba sι war le yicur thɩ̃ cʋʋ thueraakɛra n danι awι tomιra ka, dι awι khɛrsɔrakɛ thʋ̃ fi dι wa-n phɩ̃ kha khɛ haar, sι ga do thalee ti Thãgba kɔɔ ti khɛra'.
45001027	Mɛna gι ha dakha na kona, wι faarɛ mɔ̃ Thãgba tini kuun da cʋʋna khɛr, sι thue n fʋ ʋ̃ kuun na ʋ dιι ho ga hərə wer; dι wɛr kũu haar n bir gbãga na cʋʋ kha yicur thɩ̃ɛ, dι wι-n 'lɛr lιmιnɛɛkɛ teananι awι puu cʋʋra.
45001028	Dɩ mɔ̃ wa yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ teena dɩ wa hana Thãgba jɩɩra', Thãgba sɩ warɛ na awɩ kpɩɛr sɔna dɩ wa-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na teananι cʋʋra'.
45001029	Puu cʋʋ caar fɛʋ hi wer haarra, na kpallɛ, na ha pɩɛrɛ, na puu cʋʋrɛ; wɩ jɔrɛ gbugi ka, na tɩɩ kʋr, na kɩla, na fɩɩlɛ, na dakhaba cʋʋrɛ; wɩ dor lĩlirə,
45001030	na tɩɩ phiiledara, wɩ dor Thãgbaa lãlaardara, na tɩɩ nɩɩrdara, na i ƴaaldara, na nɔfa mɩɩdara, na sopugo pha cʋʋdara, na thɛ na nɛɛ nũ nʋʋrdara;
45001031	wa hana bɩ̃ kuurə', awɩ thɩmɩɩ na ha gbaarra ga, wa hana pərre dɩ wɩ jɩ tibil bʋɔra ga.
45001032	Sɩrakɛ wɩ jɩɛ jɩ dɩ Thãgba na kɩɩlnanɛ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔle, a jɩna dakha dɩ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera khir wɩ teena, sɩ ga do gɩdonɩ wɩ-n cʋʋ gɛr dɩbara ga, sɩ wo wɩ n khɩɩrɛ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera.
45002001	Dɩ fa hananakɛ thɩ̃ɛ a na ther bã, a fɩ harakɛ mɔ̃, fɛrkɛ n 'laanɛnɩ dɩ fa-n yɩ haanɩda; gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ fɩ-n 'laanɩ dɩ fa-n yɩ haanɩda, dɩbara fɩ-n heen sor, gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ fɩ-n 'laanɩ fa-n yɩɛ awɩ khara fɩ-n cʋʋ fer.
45002002	Sι jιrɛ dι Thãgbaa kιιlιkɛ a na kιιlnanι wιrɛ n cʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛ thale gι teere kha.
45002003	Fι-n kpιɛrɛ dι fɛrkɛ n 'laanɛnι dι fa-n yι wιrɛ n cʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛ thaleeda, sιι do dakha awι khara fι-n cʋʋ fa fuure Thãgbaa kιιlla gaa bɛ?
45002004	Agιbo mɔ̃ a buloni haar, a hanana jʋʋrɛ na ha fʋrɛ dιι thʋ̃ kar, fa gbarakɛ dιι do far thɩ̃a', sι fa-n ka jι dι Thãgbaa ha bulola n tɔ fι dι ga-n pɛ ha debirera ga.
45002005	Sι mɔ̃ afιda khιιrnι dι fa-n tu ha debira', Thãgbaa nĩkhi fι-n kpa fa-n thιιn gι dana nĩkhi wire, kɛ dɔnι wireekɛ Thãgbaa kιιl telẽ na ιιrnι,
45002006	dι na lιmι tιbιla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl mɔ̃ ntɛɛ thɔ̃ hanɩ.
45002007	Yire khorr a na ha wɩrɛɛkɛ n yɩranɩ dɩ wa-n cʋʋ bɔɔ, dɩ wa-n ƴaalna i dʋbɩrɛ na cʋʋrɩkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa, na gɩrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa ga.
45002008	Sɩ nĩkhii na ha helle a na lɩmɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ dɩbara nadara dɩ wɩ ka na bo sobɔr sɩ na tu dapuu.
45002009	Bɔ gaarɛ na ha dɩr na dɔ tɩbɩla ɓibiikɛ n cʋɛnɩ puureeda, Juifisɔ na dɔ cacadara, agɩpɩ wɩrɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa'.
45002010	l dʋbιrɛ, na cʋʋr, na ha ɩɩ na dɔ tibil wo tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ bɔɔda, Juifisɔra na dɔ cacadara, agɩpɩ wɩrɛ dakha na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa'.
45002011	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba na-n hɩɩn tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa'.
45002012	Ca kpala fɛʋʋkɛ n cʋɛnι sopugo sι wa jι Mʋιjιι jɔfʋa', wa bũburone na jɔfʋ 'leerera; sι Juifisɔɔkɛ hananι jɔfʋ sι wa-n cʋʋ sopugo, gιrɛ jɔfʋra n sonι na kιlɛna wι.
45002013	Gιdonι ga do wιrɛ n pɛnι jɔfʋ nũu dɔ tιι sara Thãgbara ga, sι wιrɛ n cʋɛnι gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonι sor na hɛllɔ.
45002014	Ca kpalaakɛ na hananɩ Mʋιjιι jɔfʋa', sι awι ti para wι-n cʋʋrɛ gιrɛ jɔfʋ sonι, wa hana jɔfʋ wera', sɩ awɩ thɛthɛ dɔ awɩ jɔfʋ.
45002015	Wι-n nιnanɛ dι gιrɛ jɔfʋ n ƴaalnι gι kherere awι hara, dι thalera awι kpιɛrnɔ n nιrɔ gι har, gιdonι awι kpιɛr n so warɛ aa, dapuu ha gɩrɛ aa, dabʋɔ ha gɩrɛ.
45002016	Gɛr na yɩra wireekɛ Thãgba na pɛrnɩ Jeju Kirisiti da kɩɩlna tɩbɩla awɩ thɔnaakɛ wɩ cʋʋnι wolonena, dι ga har mɔ̃kɛra tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ mι-n mιιnι sonι.
45002017	Fɛrkɛ yɛnι Juifi ha fι, dι fι bo dι fa-n ιι jɔfʋʋdara, dι fa-n məbi Thãgbaada dʋʋrra,
45002018	a jι dakha gιrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnι, jɔfʋ kɔɔ dιιr fɛr dι fι jι gιrɛ bʋɔnɔnι kpιι;
45002019	fɛrkɛ yɛnι fa marrɛ fa-n nιrɔ yara hʋɛ, aa wo, dahιrɛ fι do wιrɛraakɛ hanι dabirəra,
45002020	aa wo, də̃bələə dιιrdaar ha fι, na sikpuloosɔɔ dιιrdaar, gιdonι jɔfʋra fι jιι hana jιιr na gιrɛ dɔnι sobɔr.
45002021	Dι a mɛ̃ gι fɛrkɛ n dιrɛnι wɩ̃ tibil, fa-n dιιr afιbara gaa? Fɛrkɛ n mιanι dι fι yι wa-n yuə', fɛr n yuon?
45002022	Fɛrkɛ n sɔnι dι fι yι, tibil na-n ƴaal khɛ kpιa', tibil na-n ƴaal kũu kpιa', fɛr n ƴaalɛ khɛ kpιι? Fɛrkɛ n kpɛnι thιla, fɛr n yuon thιl du thɩ̃ɛɛ?
45002023	Fɛrkɛ n məbəni Thãgbaa jɔfʋ hananɛna, fɛr n bɔ jɔfʋ hιιnɛ dι ga-n kʋɛ Thãgbaa ii?
45002024	Mɛ̃ gι khere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Nɛr Juifisɔra n cʋɛ dι ca kpala na-n kʋɛ Thãgbaa i.”
45002025	Sobɔr gι wer, khʋ̃ kurre bɔrɛ ado fa cʋʋ gιrɛ jɔfʋ sonι, sι ado fa kʋɛ jɔfʋ afι khʋ̃ kur bire debi a ho fa kur khʋ̃a'.
45002026	Ado ʋrɛ wa kurni khʋ̃a' na cʋʋ gιrɛ jɔfʋ sonι, ga do Thãgba na-n hιιnʋʋnɛ mɔ̃ a donι khʋ̃ kurdaaraa?
45002027	Ʋrɛɛkɛrakɛ tomι nʋʋnnaakɛ na kuroni khʋ̃a', sι da-n cʋʋ gιrɛ jɔfʋ sonι na heen fι sor fɛrkɛ hananι jɔfʋ sɛbɛ na khʋ̃ kurre sι fa-n kʋɛ jɔfʋaa?
45002028	Gιdonι ga do Juifi dʋʋr tomιrra wι-n we Juifi dʋʋra', dι khʋ̃ kurre ga do tomι khʋ̃ kurreekɛ wι soa';
45002029	sι Juifi dʋʋr, bιnɔ gι ha, dι khʋ̃ kurre dʋɔn hadaa, a the Thu Phuu pa, ga do jɔfʋ sɛbɛra ga. Juifi ca olee khιι na-n the tιbιlala ga, sι Thãgbara gι-n the.
45003001	Anye Juifi dʋʋr n hana? Dɩ anyee bɔ ca khʋ̃ kurre n taa?
45003002	Thɩ̃ɛ gɩ wer waa gel. Caca thɩ̃ɛ gɩdonɩ Juifisɔ Thãgba kɔɔ dʋ ɔɔ so nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
45003003	Dɩ mɔ̃, ado ɩkhasɔ wɛrra na kɔɔ pɛr haara', mɔna wa pɛrnɩ haara' na kʋɛrɛ Thãgbaa sobɔdaar do ya?
45003004	Kpɩɩraka'. Tɩbɩla fɛʋ donɩnakɛ sõsodara, sɩ Thãgba wer sobɔ sodaarra a do, dɩ gɩ har mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ ɔɔ sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Wa yɩ fɛr dɩ fa telẽ afɩ thɩmɩɩra, fɛr na-n dɔ hʋ hanadaar kɩɩlɛlaakɛ wa-n kɩɩlna fɩnɩ.”
45003005	Dɩ ado asɩ fɩl gõgolõ na-n nɛna mɔ̃ Thãgba sarnɩ, anye sa so 'lo? Dɩ ado Thãgba gbana sɛr nĩkhii ga dor ɔɔda na saraa gaa? Tibiile mɩ mɩɩ gɩrɛ wer.
45003006	Ga ha thale kpɩɩraka'. A gɩ ha thale, mɔ̃ Thãgba na kɩɩlna tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩra?
45003007	Gɩdonɩ ado ɩ̃ sõso dɔ nɔɔ dɩ Thãgbaa sobɔ jɩɩ yɩr, a cʋʋna dakha dɩ ɔɔ i dʋbɩrɔ, mɔ̃ na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ wa kɩɩlna mɩ sopugoda dʋʋrra?
45003008	Anye na tɔna sɩ dɩ sa so nayɩ, sa-n cʋɛ puure ga-n ɩna bɔa? Thale asɩ i kʋɛdara n mɩɩ aa, sɩ sor. Wɩrɛ n mɩanɩ thale, sor na heen wer a na teena wɩ.
45003009	Dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ ha? Sɛr Juifisɔ sɩ baar wɩ̃ tibil ya? Kpei. Sɩ kɔɔ 'lire yɩ gar dɩ Juifisɔ a gbana wɩrɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa', fɛʋ sopugo n pɔtɔrɔnɛ wɩ.
45003010	Dɩ gɩ har mɔna gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Tibilikɛ saranɩ na hala', bɩɛllakɛ na hala';
45003011	tibilikɛ jɛnɩ fɩlɛ na hala', tibil bɩɛl na hale dɩ ƴaal Thãgba ga.
45003012	Fɛʋ faarɛ hʋɛ sa debi do tɩɩ kʋɛsʋsɔ ɓibi; bɩɛl na halerakɛ dɩ cʋʋ thɩ̃ bʋɔa', bιɛl 'lẽ'lenakɛ na hala'.
45003013	Awι nɔ hor mɔ̃ wι-n phuuni kaa, wι gbaar awι delẽbi dιι do fιιldaa, thιmιιrιkɛ n thɛnι awι nɔfara sikor kpalʋ gι.
45003014	Tιι nιιrɛ na thιmιι ƴʋ̃ɔ hi wer nɔɔ.
45003015	A wa ca vuu dιι do tibil wι yι ιnι-n kɔ;
45003016	awι ka pa fɛʋ, ʋʋnɛ na gaarɛ gι-n pɛ;
45003017	wa jɩ hʋɛɛkɛ n 'laanɛnɩ ha ɩɩ kpɩɩraka',
45003018	Thãgba maar na ha awɩ hara ga.”
45003019	Sɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ wɩrɛ hanɩ jɔfʋra a so, dɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na yɩ nɔ ha paara', sɩ gɩ do tɩbɩla fɛʋ sor heen wer Thãgbaa ƴɛra.
45003020	Gɩdonɩ sor na hɛl tibil bɩɛllalakɛ jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra ga, gɩdonɩ jɔfʋ n ka ɩna sopugo jɩɩr.
45003021	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ mɔ̃ Thãgba na hɛlnɩ tɩbɩlala sor, sɩ ga do jɔfʋra gɩ tha', gɩ yɩrrɛ; jɔfʋra na Thãgbaa bobonasɔ kɔɔ mɩa gɩ,
45003022	dɩ Thãgbaa so hɛlla tɩbɩlaakɛ n pɩɛrnɩ Jeju Kirisiti haar sorra n hɛllɔ, sɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar na 'lɛ, gɩdonɩ dɩɩdɩɩ hɩɩn paar na hala'.
45003023	Tɩbɩla ɓibi dʋɔn puu cʋʋdara a 'lee i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaada.
45003024	Sɩ khaar sor na hɛl war ɔɔ bɔ jɩra gɩ the birsereraakɛ Jeju Kirisiti birse wini.
45003025	Dɩ ɔr Thãgba gba a jinə bonɩɛ dɩ ɔɔ tɔmɩ̃ na do sopugo hɛldaa wɩrɛraakɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar, gɩ nɩna ɔɔ fɩl sar, gɩdonɩ aa kɔɔ therna sopugookɛ tɩbɩla kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ mamara ɔɔ ha fʋ bɔra ga.
45003026	Sɩ a ƴaalɛ a nɩna ɔɔ fɩl sar nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛ, gɛr na nɛna dɩ ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ saranɩ da-n hɛl ʋrɛ n pɩɛrnɩ Jeju haar sor.
45003027	Dɩ kana gɩrɛ tibil na məbironi ha? Ga hala'. Anye dɔ nɔɔ? Jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛ dɔ nɔɔ ya? Kpei. Ha pɛrɛra gɩ the.
45003028	Gɩdonɩ sɩ yɩ gɛr dɩ ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ tibil n 'lɛrɔ so hɛllɛ, ga do jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra ga.
45003029	Dɩ Thãgbara, Juifisɔɔ Thãgba a ba do dɩbara ya? Ga do ca kpalaa Thãgba a do dakha gaa? Ɔɔ, ca kpalaa Thãgba a do dakha.
45003030	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba bɩɛlla a do, dɩ cʋʋ sor dɩ ga-n hɛl khʋ̃ kurdarara dɩɩ the awɩ ha pɛra, dɩ cʋʋ sor dɩ ga-n hɛl wɩrɛraakɛ na kuroni khʋ̃a', dɩɩ do ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ.
45003031	Dɩ ha pɛrɛ ba dor nɔɔ dɩ sɩ cʋʋrɔ jɔfʋ dιι debi a do mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ ya? Kpιιraka'. Jɔfʋ sι ka jιι cʋʋ dɩɩ do jɔfʋ.
45004001	A mɛ̃ gɩ, mɔ̃ sa so Abɩrahamnaakɛ dɔnɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃? Anye a kɔɔ 'lɛ na ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ fãga?
45004002	Ado sor kɔɔ hɛllɛ Abɩrahamna dɩɩ the thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra a hananɛ gɩrɛ a na məbironi, sɩ ga do Thãgbaa ƴɛra ga.
45004003	Gɩdonɩ anye Thãgbaa sɛbɛ so? Gɩ sor: “Abɩraham kɔɔ pɛr Thãgba haar dɩɩ do gɛr Thãgba hɩɩn sa wɩɩ tɩɩ sarʋ.”
45004004	Mee ʋrɛ dɔnɩ thɔma wɩ-n lɩmʋʋnɛ, ga do khaardaa wa hɩɩn gɩ gɩ dora', sɩ helu gɩ dɩ wɩ lɩmʋʋ.
45004005	Sɩ ʋrɛ na-n cʋɛnɩ thɩ̃a', sɩ dɩ pɛr haar ʋrɛraakɛ n hɛlanɩ sopugodaarra sor, Thãgba na thernanɛ ɔɔ ha pɛɛle dɩ sor na hɛllaa.
45004006	Mɛ̃ Davɩdɩ mɩɩ mɔ̃ ga danɩ tibilləəkɛ Thãgba n hɛllɔnɩ sor sɩ ga-n the thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra ga, ayɩ:
45004007	“Gɩ-n dar wɩrɛraakɛ Thãgba faanɩ awɩ dakhaba do, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ dakha a hɛllɔnɩ sopugo.
45004008	Gɩ-n dar tibilləəkɛ Kɔ̃tɩn na-n thernɩ ɔɔ sopugo da-n ha ga.”
45004009	Dɩ ga kãka caakɛra khʋ̃ kurdaraada gɩ do dɩbara yaa, agɩbo wɩrɛ na kuroni khʋ̃aada gɩ do dakha? Gɩdonɩ sɩ kɔɔ sor ayɩ: “Abιrahamι ha pɛ dɔ nɔɔ dι Thãgba wιι tιι sarʋ.”
45004010	Dι bɔ ʋmɔna gι? Ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ kurni khʋ̃ʋ gι yaa, agιbo ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ kurni khʋ̃ʋ paa gι? Ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ kurni khʋ̃ʋ paa gι, dι a dor ʋrɛ na kɔɔ kuroni khʋ̃a'.
45004011	A kɔɔ 'lɛr jιιnιkɛ dɔnι khʋ̃ kurdaa dɩɩ do gɛr n nɛna so hɛllɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ ha pɛrɛra, ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ kurni khʋ̃a'; dɩ mɛ̃ a do thɩrɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar, kɛ na kuroni khʋ̃a', dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba n hɩɩn wɩ dɩ wɩ do fɩl sardara.
45004012	Abɩraham dor thɩrɛ dakha khʋ̃ kurdarara, sɩ ga do khʋ̃ kurdara ha wɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ wɛr dɔ wɩrɛɛkɛ n kpaannɩ asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abɩrahamɩ ha pɛraakɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ kurni khʋ̃ʋ pa'.
45004013	Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛrɛ ayɩ, Abɩraham na ɔɔ məlsɔ na hɩna thɩɩkɛ; dɩ ga do jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ Thãgba ʋlfɛnaa thala', sɩ ha pɛrɛɛkɛ a hananɩ a 'lɛrɔ so hɛllɛ dɔ nɔɔ.
45004014	Gɩdonɩ ado jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ wɩ do thɩ̃ hɩna, ga dor ha pɛrɛ wer mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ gɩ, dɩ ʋlfɛrɛ dakha kʋkʋʋlɛ.
45004015	Gɩdonɩ jɔfʋ n ɩrɛna Thãgbaa nĩkhi, dɩ ka jɔfʋ na-n hana', jɔfʋ kʋɛrɛ na-n hale dakha ga.
45004016	Mɛ̃ thɩ̃ hɩ̃ 'lɛrɩle the ha pɛrɛra gɩ do bɔ jɩɩrra gɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ ʋlfɛrɛɛle na puno phubi a na do Abɩrahamɩ məl fɛʋʋda, sɩ ga do ɔɔ məlikɛ dɔnɩ jɔfʋdara dɩbara ga, sɩ gɩ do wɩrɛ fɛʋ hananɩ Abɩrahamɩ ha pɛɛda; gɩdonɩ Abɩraham dʋɔn sɛrɛ fɛʋʋ thɩ.
45004017	Dɩ gɩ har mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Mɩ thɩɩn fɛr fɩ do ca jɔɔ thɩ.” A do sarɛ thɩrɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ a pɛrnɩ haar, kɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaakɛ n cʋɛnɩ khe dɩ wɩ bir hana yire, dɩ gɩrɛ na hanɩle pa' sɩ a-n therna gɛr mɔ̃kɛ gɩ hanɩle.
45004018	Abɩraham hananɛ ha pɛrɛ Thãgbara gɛr gɩ dɩ hana nũ pɛrɛ gɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ dacʋʋnaa ga, dɩ mɛ̃ a debi a do “ca jɔɔ thɩ”, dɩ gɩ har mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba sonɩ ayɩ: “Thale afɩ məl na ha.”
45004019	Ɔɔ ha pɛɛkɛ a hananɩ ga wurə', sɩrakɛ yɛna tamaa a kɔɔ thɔɔ a dã khir, dɩ Saraa bi kɔ̃ bɔ dakha 'li kar.
45004020	Sɩ ha pɛrɛ na ɓɔrʋa', dɩ aa-n baal Thãgbaa ʋlfɛra woa', sɩ ha pɛrɛ cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ 'lɛ fãga da-n khɩɩ Thãgba.
45004021	A hananɛ tu jɩɩr gel dɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba ʋlfɛnɩ ɩna cʋʋrɛ a na puno ger a na cʋʋ;
45004022	dɩ gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dɩ “Thãgba wɩɩ tɩɩ sarʋ.”
45004023	Thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ kherenenɩ ayɩ, “Thãgba wɩɩrɛ tɩɩ sarʋ”, ga do ɔr dɩbara gɩ soa'.
45004024	Sɩ sɩ harrɛ ser tɩɩ sar dʋʋrraale, sɛrkɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar ʋrɛraakɛ ɩrɛnɩ Jeju asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ dɩ the khirera.
45004025	Ʋrɛɛkɛ wɩ kʋnɩ asɩ sopugora sɩ dɩ ɩɩr a the khirera sor n hɛl sar.
45005001	Dɩ mɔ̃ Thãgba hɛl sarnɩ sor thakɛ dɩɩ do ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ, sɩ hananɛ ha ɩɩ na ɔr dɩɩ the Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩna.
45005002	Ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sɩ ba yɩrɔ ha pɛrɛra lõ paar bɔ jɩ caarraakɛ sɩ jɩɩlɔnɩ gɩrɛ kɩbɩ, dɩ sa-n kãka nũ pɛrɛraakɛ sɩ hananɩ a na bul kha na Thãgbaa i dʋbɩ.
45005003	Dɩrakɛ wo sɩ-n kãkarɛ bɔ gaarɛra gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ bɔ gaarɛ n ɛna ha fʋrɛ,
45005004	dɩ ha fʋrɛɛle na cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sa for a na bɩ̃, dɩ bɩɩnɩle n 'laanɛ nũ pɛrɛ.
45005005	Dɩ nũ pɛrɛɛle na pɛ sar yicuruə', gɩdonɩ naʋʋkɛ Thãgba na sɩnɩ gɩ və̃viəne a hi asɩ hara, dɩ Thu Phuu pa gɩ the, kɛ Thãgba ha sɩnɩ.
45005006	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sa-n kɔɔ yɩrɔnɩ fɛfɛɛ paar kpɩɩa', gɛr Kirisiti khiro sɛr sopugodarara, bɔɔkɛ Thãgba pɛrnɩ danɩ.
45005007	Dɩ fa tee tɩɩ sarʋʋ khi a na khi gɩ khɩɩrɛ, sɩ anaa ʋkha na ture a na tee tɩɩ bʋɔɔ khi a na khi.
45005008	Sɩ yɛ gɩrɛ n nɛnanɩ mɔ̃ Thãgbaa naʋʋkɛ a na sɩnɩ hanɩ: Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ donɩ sopugodara 'lo gɛr Kirisiti ka khiro asɩ sora.
45005009	Dɩ mɔ̃ ga ka na ha gɩrɛ dɩphã ɔɔ tɔmɩ̃ hɛl sɩnɩ sor, gɩ do aa ka taa sɩ Thãgbaa nĩkhirə ga.
45005010	Gɩdonɩ ado ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ donɩ lãlaardara na Thãgba, ɔɔ Bikuuni khi cʋʋ sɛr dɩ sɩ bir kũu kha na Thãgba; dɩ mɔ̃ ga ka na ha gɩrɛ dɩphã sɩ birni kũu kha na Thãgba gɩ do Kirisitii yi na taa sa'.
45005011	Sɩ ga do gele gɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ dakha sɩ-n kãkarɛ Thãgbara dɩɩ the asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira ʋrɛɛkɛra sɩ 'lɛrnɩ bir kuune dɩphã.
45005012	Nɩ yɛ mɔ̃ gɩ hanɩ: Tibil bɩɛl dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sopugo ba lona thɩɩra, dɩ sopugorara khir the, dɩ khirrə mar tɩbɩla ɓibi, gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla ɓibi n cʋɛ sopugo.
45005013	Sopugo kɔɔ 'lire hakɛ thɩɩra sɩ dɩ jɔfʋ pɩɩrɔ 'laa, sɩ kãkɛ jɔfʋ na hana', sopugo therre na hala'.
45005014	Dɩ a fʋna Adãa bɔɔ a dana Mʋɩjɩɩ bɔɔ khir n punone tɩbɩla fɛʋ, narakɛ wɩrɛ na kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ sopugo Thãgbara dɩɩ ho Adãada ga; dɩ Adana hʋɔn ʋrɛ na ɩnanɩ.
45005015	Sɩ bʋɔraakɛ Thãgba n jɩnɩ tibil dɩɩ do khaardaa gɩ do, gɩ har kpɩɩ na sopugo. Gɩdonɩ tɩɩ bɩɛlɩ sopugo dor nɔɔ dɩ tɩɩ jɔjʋɔ khiir, sɩ bʋɔraakɛ Thãgba n jɩnɩ tibil na khaardaakɛ a-n 'laanɩ pɔɩ dɩɩ do tɩɩ bɩɛlɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ, gɩ kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ gele fɩ̃i a ƴɛr a dã tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
45005016	Thãgbaa khaarda na gɩrɛ tibili sopugo cʋʋnɩ gɩ har dɩɩdɩɩ: Sopugo bɩɛl dɩbara gɛr ɩrɛna kɩɩlʋ dɩ sor heen tɩbɩla gɩrɛ, sɩ sopugo jɔjʋɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla cʋʋnɩ sor ka hɛl warɛ dɩɩ do bɔ jɩ khaardaa dɔ nɔɔ.
45005017	Ado tibil bɩɛlɩ sopugo do nɔɔ dι khir na-n puno tɩbɩla fɛʋ dɩɩ the tɩɩ bɩɛllaalera, mɔ̃ gɩrɛ tɩɩ bɩɛlɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ cʋʋnι na thʋ̃ na ha? Gɛr dʋɔn wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ 'lɛnι Thãgbaa bɔ jι jɔɔ na khaardaakɛ dɔnι so hɛllɛ, na dor punodara awι yi hanana gι do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
45005018	Gɛr gι mɔ̃kɛ tιι bιɛlι sopugo donι nɔɔ dι so heene dã tɩbɩla fɛʋ, ɔmɛna tɩɩ bɩɛlι fιl sar thɔ̃ na cuu tɩbɩla fɛu dɩ sor na hɛl war dɩ wa 'lɛ yire.
45005019	Mɔ̃kɛ tɩɩ bɩɛlɩ nũ nʋʋr cʋʋnɩ tɩbɩla jɔɔ dɩ wɩ do sopugodara, mɛ̃ tɩɩ bɩɛlɩ nũ nɩ na cʋʋ tɩbɩla jɔɔ dɩ sor na hɛl war.
45005020	Jɔfʋ 'lɔɔrɔrɛ gɩ cʋʋ sopugo gι jɔr, dι ka sopugo jɔrnι le Thãgbaa bɔ jι n jιι jɔr.
45005021	Mɛ̃ gɩɩ, mɔna sopugo punoni tɩbɩla fɛʋ da-n 'laa khir, mɛ̃ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ dakha hana punone dɩ ga-n hɛl tɩbɩlala sor gɩ kpa sɩ gɩ pɛ yire khorra, gɩ do Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ pa gɩ the.
45006001	Dɩ mɔ̃ sa so gɩrɛ? Sa-n cʋɛ sopugo bɔ jɩɩrra na-n jɩɩ jɔr ya?
45006002	Kpɩɩraka'. Sɛrkɛ khenɩ sopugo cʋʋrɛra, anyee yi ca sa hana sopugo cʋʋrɛra 'lo?
45006003	Na jɩ dɩɩ do sɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpɛɛnɩ nyʋɔnɔ bɩɛl dʋʋrra nakha Jeju Kirisiti, bιɛl dʋʋrra nakha ɔɔ khi wɩ kɔɔ kpɛɛ saa?
45006004	Mɛ̃ gι yɔ kpɛɛrɛ dʋɔn wι dʋ sɛr kha na ɔr mɔ̃ sι khini kha, dι mɔ̃kɛ Thιrɛɛ fãga kɔɔ ιιrnι Kirisiti dι the khirera, sɛrɛ dakha yi phaara sa-n ιιrna oti.
45006005	Gιdonι ado sι debire a do kha bιɛl na ɔr khirraakɛ hɔnι ɔɔda, sa debire dakha a na do bιɛl na ɔr ɔɔ khi ιιrra.
45006006	Sι jι gɛr dι tιι tɩ̃ dʋʋrιkɛ sι kɔɔ donι wι kɔɔ kpaarɛ kʋkʋ thιrʋra nakha Kirisiti, gι do nɔɔ asι mɛrɛ puurə n kʋkʋʋl, dι mɛ̃ sa do sopugoo deesɔ bã.
45006007	Gιdonι ʋrɛ khenɩ a ther sopugoo nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
45006008	Dɩ ado sɩ kɔɔ khire ger nakha Kirisiti, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sa hananɛ kha yire na ɔr.
45006009	Gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ Kirisiti kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a the khirera dɩ khir na punoo bã.
45006010	Khirikɛ a kɔɔ khini sopugo a kɔɔ khiro babɩɛl dɩbara dɩɩ do gɩ daan, sɩ yireekɛ a hananɩ nɛnɛ̃ Thãgbara a hana gɩ.
45006011	Mɛ̃ gɩ, nɛrɛ dakha, na-n hɩnɛ dɩbara mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ khe sopugo cʋʋrɛra sa do yidara Thãgbara dɩɩ the anɩ bɩɛl dora na Jeju Kirisiti.
45006012	Na-n do sopugo na-n puno anɩ tomɩ khinəəkɛ nɩ nɩɩ nũu na-n cʋʋ gɩrɛ n kʋɔnɩ thueə'.
45006013	Na-n gba anɩ tomɩ ɓãsɔ 'lo a faa sopugo cʋʋrɛra gɩ do fɩl gõgolõ thɔ̃ dodaa ga; sɩ nɩ faa anɩbara Thãgbara mɔ̃kɛ nɩ donɩ wɩrɛ khenɩ sa ɩɩr a the khirera, nɩ gba anɩ tomɩ ɓãsɔ a na hana Thãgba a na-n cʋʋna gɩrɛ saranɩ.
45006014	Gɩdonɩ sopugo na-n pɔtɔrɔ nɩ bã, gɩdonɩ ga do jɔfʋra nɩ ha ga, sɩɩ do Thãgbaa bɔ jɩra gɩ.
45006015	Dɩ mɔ̃ ga ha? Sa-n cʋɛ sopugo gɩdonɩ ga do jɔfʋra sɩ ha ga sɩɩ do bɔ jɩɩrra gɩ ya? Kpɩɩraka'.
45006016	Na jɩ dɩɩ do a fɩ faa afɩbara tibillə a do dee fa-n nɩɩ nũu, ga do ʋrɛɛkɛɛ nũ fɩ-n nɩnɩ ɔɔ dee fɩ doaa, a sopugo fɩ-n nɩ nũu khirrə ga jalna fι, a Thãgba fι-n nι nũu sor a na hɛl far.
45006017	Thãgba hιna fʋɔrɛ. Nɛrɛɛkɛ mamara kɔɔ dɔnι sopugoo deesɔ, nι bire a nι nũu na haar fɛʋ dιιr caaraakɛ nι kɔɔ 'lɛnι.
45006018	Nɛnɛ̃ Thãgba birse ner sopugo dee dʋʋrra dι nι debi a do Thãgbaa deesɔ dι na-n cʋʋ gιrɛ saranι.
45006019	Tibiile mι mιι gιdonι ka nι hanι gιrɛ nι yɔɔrɛ; mɔ̃ nι kɔɔ faanι anι tomι ɓãsɔ a do dea thɩ̃ bise cʋʋrɛra na sopugora gι jιι jɔr, nɛnɛ̃ nι faa anι tomι ɓãsɔ ɔmɛ̃ a dɔ Thãgbaa deesɔ a na cʋɛ gιrɛ saranι a dana kpιι leere.
45006020	Gιdonι ɔbɔɔkɛ nι kɔɔ donι sopugoo deesɔ na ha kha dιkha na fιl sarʋa'.
45006021	Gιmɔ̃ dɔ khor nι kɔɔ 'lɛrnι ɔbɔɔraalera? Gɛr dɔ gιrɛ cʋɛnι dι yicuru na-n fʋ nι nɛnɛ̃kɛ, gιdonι ga khu pa dʋɔn khir.
45006022	Sι nɛnɛ̃kɛ Thãgba birse ner sopugo dee dʋʋrra a cʋʋ nι dι nι do ɔɔ deesɔ, dι kpιι leere dʋɔn anιda sι khu paar n do yire khorr.
45006023	Gιdonι lιmιnɛɛkɛ sopugo n lɩmɩnɩ khir gɩ, sɩ khaardaakɛ Thãgba n 'laanɩ pɔɩ, gɛr dʋɔn yire khorr, kɛ hanɩ Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩna.
45007001	Nɛr omɩnaakɛ dɔnɩ jɔfʋ jɩna mɩ-n mɩɩna, na jɩ dɩɩ do bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ tibil hananι yire gɛr jɔfʋ n punonaa dιbara gaa?
45007002	Mɛ̃ jɔfʋ n li khɛr na ɔɔ ko bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ kuun hananι yire, sι a kuun khi pι, khɛr n ther jɔfʋraakɛ lieni kha na ɔɔ ko.
45007003	Sι ado bɔɔkɛ ɔɔ ko hananι yire, gɛr khɛr biro a ma kũu kpιι, kũu kpιι ƴaaldaar wa-n we khɛrιle; sι ado ɔɔ ko khe, khɛrιle na ha kha dιkha na jɔfʋ bã, a a debi do kũu kpιι khɛr ga do kũu kpιι ƴaaldaar a doa'.
45007004	Mɛ̃ gι ha na nɛrɛ ɩ̃ omisɔ; nɛrɛ dakha nι kɔɔ khire jɔfʋdaara dιι the anι bιɛl dora na Kirisiti nι fi nι do tιι kpιιda, ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ ιrɛnι a the khirera gι, sι puno sa-n se be Thãgbara.
45007005	Gιdonι ɔbɔɔkɛ sι-n kɔɔ ιιrnι a ho tibil ba, sopugoo ƴaalιkɛ jɔfʋ cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ hale n kɔɔ dor thɔma asɩ tomɩ ɓãsɔra dɩɩ do khir gɩ-n ɩna sar.
45007006	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ sɩ ther jɔfʋraakɛ kɔɔ le sɩnɩ mɔ̃ sɩ khini gɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ fɔ sɩnɩ ɩɩrɔ, gɩ do nɔɔ sa-n do thɔma Thãgbara na fɩl phaakɛ Thu Phuu n thɔɔna sɩnɩ, ga ha mɔ̃ datɩ̃ɩ hanɩ kɛ dɔnɩ jɔfʋʋdaakɛ kherenena'.
45007007	Dɩ mɔ̃ sa so gɩrɛ? Jɔfʋ dʋɔn sopugo ya? Kpɩɩraka'. Sɩ jɔfʋ cʋɛ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ jɩ thɩ̃ doo n dɔnɩ sopugo; gɩdonɩ ma kɔɔ jɩ thĩ doo n dɔnɩ ha pɩɛrɛ ado jɔfʋ na kɔɔ so ayɩ, fa-n Pɩɛr hara gaaga.
45007008	Dɩ jɔfʋ dor nɔɔ dɩ sopugo yɩrɔ hʋɛ a cʋʋ ha pɩɛr caar fɛʋ dɩɩ ɩɩr mar, gɩdonɩ ado jɔfʋ na hala', ga dor thĩ khire sopugo do.
45007009	Mɛrɛ mɩ kɔɔ hananɛ yire bɔɔraakɛ ma kɔɔ hananɩ jɔfʋ pa', sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ jɔfʋ ɩnɩ, gɛr sopugo ɩɩrɔ vuu dɩɩ do mɩ khire.
45007010	Dɩ jɔfʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ yi 'laadaa fire a do mar khi 'laadaa.
45007011	Gɩdonɩ sopugo yɩrɛ hʋɛ da-n fɩɩl mɩ dɩɩ do jɔfʋʋ pa gɩ the, dɩ a gbaar jɔfʋʋlera a kʋna mɩ.
45007012	Thãgbaa jɔfʋsɔ wer phure, dɩ jɔfʋ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl phure, a sar, a bɔrna.
45007013	Dɩ gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ fire a do mar khir kɛ? Kpɩɩraka', sɩ sopugo gɩ; mɛ̃ sopugo nɩna mɔ̃ a jɩɩnɩ do sopugo mɔ̃ a gbanɩ gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ dɩɩ fi do mar khir; mɛ̃ jɔfʋ do nɔɔ dɩ sopugo debi a jɩɩ puuro a pɛr.
45007014	Sɩ jɩrɛ wer dɩ thudaa jɔfʋ do, sɩ mɛrɛ tibil ha mɩ na tomɩr dɩ ɩ̃ dona sopugoo dee.
45007015	Ma jɩ ɩ̃ cʋʋ pa tɔrrakɛ mɔ̃ gɩ hana', ga do gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ ɩ̃ cʋɛ gɛr mɩ-n cʋa', sɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n laarnɩ khələlələ gɛr mɩ-n ka cʋʋ.
45007016	Ado gɩrɛ ma-n ƴaalnɩ ɩ̃ cʋa' gɛr mɩ-n cʋʋ, thale n nɛna dɩ mɩ ture dɩ jɔfʋ bɔrɛ.
45007017	Dɩ a thɩɛna gaa ga do mɛr n cʋ ga, sɩ sopugookɛ hanɩ ɩ̃ hara n cʋɛ.
45007018	Gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩrɛ thɩ̃ bʋɔ na ha ɩ̃ bɩnɔa', a thɩɛna gaa ɩ̃ tibil do para; thɩ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛɛ ƴaal wer har ɩ̃ hara, sɩ punone na hala'.
45007019	Ma-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ bʋɔɔkɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ ɩ̃ cʋa', sɩ puureekɛ ma-n kanɩ ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋa' dɩɩ do gɛr mɩ-n cʋʋ.
45007020	Dɩ ado ma cʋʋ gɩrɛ ma-n ƴaalnɩ ɩ̃ cʋa', ga do mɛr ɩ̃ eʋ ga sɩ sopugookɛ hanɩ ɩ̃ hara n cʋɛ.
45007021	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ mι yιnι ɩ̃ pa dʋɔn: A mι yι bɔɔ mι ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋʋ sι puure na-n ha mι thɩ̃ thaa ga.
45007022	Ado bιnɔ wer gι, Thãgbaa jɔfʋ da marɛ haar ka,
45007023	sι a mι gba na hɩɩn ɩ̃ tomɩ ɓãsɔ dɩɩ do thɩ̃ kpɩɩ hale n kɛ̃kɛrɛnanɩ gɩrɛ ɩ̃ ha yɩnɩ dabʋɔ gɩ, dɩ thɩ̃ɛɛlera dʋɔn sopugoo jɔfʋ a pɛrnɩ dɩɩ ha ɩ̃ tomι ɓãsɔra dι ɩ̃ fi do dee.
45007024	Pha, mɛr bɔ kʋ tibilikɛ, amɛ na taa mι na ti mi tomɩ khinənenaakɛ?
45007025	Thãgba hɩna fʋɔrɛ, gɩdonɩ Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ pa taarɛ na the. Gɛr gɩ, me wer haarra Thãgbaa jɔfʋʋ dee mɩ do, sι ɩ̃ tibil do para dee mι do sopugoo jɔfʋra.
45008001	Nɛnɛ̃ gɩrɛ so heene na hale kpɩɩrakɛ wɩrɛraakɛ hanɩ Jeju Kirisitira ga.
45008002	Gɩdonɩ Thu Phuu fãgaakɛ n 'laanɛnɩ yire dɩɩ the asɩ bɩɛl dora nakha Jeju Kirisiti, gɛr birsene mi a ti mi sopugoo fãgara na khiri fãgara.
45008003	Gɩrɛ jɔfʋ na kɔɔ punoni a cʋa', gɩdonɩ tibili tibil do pa a 'leere fãga, Thãgba kɔɔ cʋʋ gɛr, gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ thʋɔn ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ Bikuun dɩɩ do sopugo dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ gba tibil tomɩr dɩɩ hona asɩ sopugo tomɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba heen sopugookɛ hanɩ tibili tibil do para sor.
45008004	Thãgba cʋʋrɛ gele dι mɛ̃ sɛrɛɛkɛ na-n ιrɛnι mɔ̃kɛ asι tibil do pa n ƴaalna', sιι do mɔ̃ Thu Phuu n ƴaalnι sι-n ιιr, na cʋʋ datelẽekɛ jɔfʋ n ƴaalnι ga-n cʋɛ.
45008005	Gιdonι wιrɛ n ιrɛnι na tibil dʋʋrιkɛ fãga 'leenι, awι kpιɛr koo tibili tibil do padara gι-n jal; sι wιrɛ n ιrɛnι mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuu n so warnι, awι kpιɛr koo Thu Phuudarara gι-n jal.
45008006	Kpιɛr faarɛ koo tibili tibil do padara khir gι, sι kpιɛr faarɛ koo Thu Phuudara yire gι na ha ιι.
45008007	Gιdonι kpιɛr faarɛ koo tibili tibil do padara, gι-n ιnanɛ laarɛ nakha Thãgba; gιdonι tibili tibil do pa na-n wur dιbara Thãgbaa jɔfʋra ga, dι a na puno gιrakɛ dakha ga.
45008008	Dι wιrɛɛkɛ n ιrɛnι na tibil dʋʋrɩkɛ fãga 'leenɩ wa puno na da Thãgba haarra ga.
45008009	Sɩ ne wer na-n ɩɩr na tibil dʋʋrιkɛ fãga 'leena', sι mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuu n so narnι nι-n ιιr, adora Thãgbaa Thu har anι bιnɔ. Ado tibil na hana Kirisitii Thuə', aa do Kirisitiida ga.
45008010	Ado Kirisiti har anι bιnɔ, sιrakɛ dιι do anι tomι khire dιι do sopugo dɔ nɔɔ, sι thue na hananɛ yire gι do so hɛllɛ dɔ nɔɔ.
45008011	Ado Thãgbaa Thuukɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnι Jeju dι ιιr a the khirera ha anι bιnɔ, ʋrɛɛkɛra cʋɛnι Jeju Kirisiti dι ιιr a the khirera, ɔrra na 'laanɛ yire anι tomι khinəna, gι the ɔɔ Thurəəkɛra hanι anι bιnɔ.
45008012	Gɛr gι omιna, sι hananɛ helu sι ga do asι tibil do pa sι hana helu sa-n ιιr mɔ̃kɛ a-n ƴaalna'.
45008013	Ado na ιιr mɔ̃kɛ tibili tibil do pa n ƴaalnι khir nι fʋ fʋrɔ, sι ado Thu Phuu nι-n ka gba dι na-n kʋna gιrɛ tibili tibil do pa n cʋʋnι ga dor na hananɛ yire.
45008014	Gιdonι wιrɛɛkɛ n pɛnι Thãgbaa Thu nũu, wɛr dɔ Thãgbaa bikuunsɔ.
45008015	Gιdonι Thu Phuukɛ nι 'lɛnι ga cʋʋ nɩ nɩ ho dea nɩ bir nɩ lõ maarra ga, sɩ Thu Phuukɛ cʋɛ nɩnɩ dɩ nɩ do Thãgbaa bikuunsɔ gɩ, dɩ sa-n wero: Aba, ɩ̃ Thɩ.
45008016	Thu Phuu thɛthɛ n gbɛba kha na asɩ thu sɩ da-n nɩrɔ dɩ sɩ dor Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔ.
45008017	Dɩ ado ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ sɩ do, sɩ dor dakha thɩ̃ hɩna; Thãgbaa thɩ̃ hɩ̃dara ha sɩ, dɩ sɩ bul kha na Kirisiti thɩ̃ɛ a hɩ̃, adora sɩ-n gaarɛ bʋɔ na ɔr gɩ do nɔɔ sɩ gbɛbɩ kha na ɔɔ i dʋbɩ.
45008018	Mɩ jɩrɛ tue dɩ bʋɔɔkɛ sɩ-n gaarnɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ, ga hɩɩr kha na i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgba na ha sɩna'.
45008019	Thɩ̃ tinəne koo n pɩɛrɛ gɩrɛ na ƴaal kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ka bɔɔkɛ Thãgba na nɩrɔnɩ ɔɔ bikuunsɔ.
45008020	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ fɔnɩ thɩ̃ tinəne a ɩɩrɔ dɩɩ debi a do mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ, ga do gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ tinəne ƴaalɛ gɛr a cʋʋrɔ mã';
45008021	sɩ gɩ do nũ pɛrɛ hale, dɩ thɩ̃ tinənee thɛthɛra na ther kʋɛ dee dʋʋrra a na lõ Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔɔ wa doraakɛ na ɓɔnanɩ na ka.
45008022	Gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ thɩ̃ tinəne ɓibi n ser da-n gaarna a ho mɔ̃ wallɛ n fʋnɩ khɛr.
45008023	Ga do thɩ̃ tinəne bɩɛl gɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ na sɛrɛ dakharakɛ, kɛ hananɩ Thu Phuu dɩ do caca khaardaa ɓo, sɩ-n ser ser na bɩnɛ, dɩ sa-n pɩɛrna bikũu dʋʋr na asɩ tomɩ birse.
45008024	Gɩdonɩ asɩ taakɛ sɩ 'lɛnɩ nũ pɛrɛra gɩ do; sɩ a sɩ yɩ gɩrɛ sɩ-n pɛnɩ nũu pι na yire, ga do nũ pɛrɛ gι bã; gιdonι amɛ na-n pɛ nũu gιrɛraakɛ a yιnι pι?
45008025	Sι ado sa pɛ nũu gιrɛraakɛ sa yιna', mee ha fʋrɛ sa-n pιɛrna thɩ̃ doole.
45008026	Mɛ̃ dakha Thu Phuu n bul si asι yɔɔra, gιdonι sa-n jιι jι mɔ̃ sa bιɛlnι na gιrɛ teananι bιɛla', sι Thu Phuu thɛthɛ har da-n phʋʋr Thãgba na 'wιιrɛɛkɛ na hanι mιιrɛra ga.
45008027	Dι ʋrɛɛkɛ n bəəreni tibili bɩ̃ dι jι, ɔr jιɛn gιrɛ dɔnι Thu Phuu kpιɛrnɔ, gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni a-n phʋʋr Thãgba da-n pɛr tibil phuusɔ.
45008028	Sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ Thãgba n cʋɛ dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ n kpalmã dɩɩ fi, a do dabʋɔ wɩrɛraakɛ n naanɛɛnɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ a kɔɔ wenɩ mɔ̃ ɔɔ ƴaal hanɩ.
45008029	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ a kɔɔ maanɩ jɩɩr a kɔɔ mãa phiir war dɩ wa debi na ha mɔ̃ ɔɔ Bikuun hanɩ, gɩ do mɛ̃ Bikuunile do cacadaar omɩna bərəəmna.
45008030	Dɩ welela a kɔɔ maanɩ phiire, wɛr dɔ wɩrɛ a wenɩ, dɩ wɩrɛra a wenɩ wɛr dɔ wɩrɛ sor hɛllɔnɩ, dɩ wɩrɛ a hɛllɔnɩ sorra wɩ lʋʋn dakha ɔɔ i dʋbιra.
45008031	Dι thɩ̃ɛ hanι thakɛ anye sa so 'lo? Ado sɛr Thãgba hana amɛ na punone na ma sar?
45008032	Ɔrkɛ na kɔɔ tɔnanι ɔɔ Bikuuna' sιι do a fagʋʋrɛ sɛrɛ fɛʋʋ sora, dɩ mɔ̃ ga fʋ sɩɩ do aa ka ha sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ khaar a ɓaana?
45008033	Amɛ na pɩɛr wɩrɛ Thãgba phiirni sor? Mee Thãgba n hɛla sor.
45008034	Dɩ amɛ na heene tibil sor? Wa bɩɛl na hala'. Jeju Kirisiti ka kɔɔ khire sɩ ga do gele gɩ koa', a ɩɩrɛ a the khirera, a ha dakha gɩrɛ Thãgbaa nyɔ̃bɔra, da-n phʋʋr Thãgba da-n pɛ sar.
45008035	Dɩ amɛ na lea sɩ na Kirisitii naʋʋkɛ a-n na sɩnɩ? Bɔ gaarɛ na punone ya? Sɩ nɩwɛ, agɩbo kpoore, sɩ kɔmɛr, sɩ bʋɔ, sɩ khi phuronaa, sɩ bajɩna? Kpɩɩraka'.
45008036	Sɩ gɩ har mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Fɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sɩ too khikhi togʋʋ dɩwɩlʋ koo; wɩ-n hɩɩn sɛr mɔ̃ sɩ donɩ banaakɛ wa kʋʋrnɩ.”
45008037	Sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋraakɛ sɩ kəə garɛ fii dɩɩ the ʋrɛ kɔɔ naan sɩnɩɩ pa.
45008038	Gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩɛ jɩ tue dɩ thɩ̃ɛ na hale a na puno na lee sɩ kha na ɔɔ naʋa': A khir gɩ, a yi hananɛ gɩ, a thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ wɛ, a fãga hɩ̃darasɔ wɛ ƴũ, a thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hanɩ nɛnɛ̃ gɩrɛ gɩ, a gɩrɛ na ɩnanɩ gɩ,
45008039	a punoneekɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ a tɩɛr gɩ, thɩ̃ bɩɛl na halerakɛ thɩ̃ tinəne fɛʋra a na puno kpɩɩrakɛ a na lee sɩ na Thãgbaa naʋʋkɛ a na sɩnɩ dɩɩ the Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ pa ga.
45009001	Sobɔr mɩ-n so mɔ̃ mɩ donɩ Kirisitiida, ma-n sõsoa'. Ɩ̃ kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ n pɛnɩ Thu Phuuda nũu yɩ gɛr dɩ sobɔr mɩ-n so,
45009002	dɩ gbobire jɔɔ na ha helle n har ɩ̃ hara wire fɛʋ.
45009003	Dɩ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ ka nar sʋɔn n 'le mɩ gɩ lee mɩ kpɩɩ nakha Kirisiti ɩ̃ omisɔɔ sora, kɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ ca bɩnɔ,
45009004	kɛ dɔnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldara, kɛ Thãgba cʋʋnɩ dɩ wɩ do ɔɔ bikuunsɔ, a dona wɩrɛ a cʋʋnɩ dɩ wɩ jɩ mɔ̃ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ hanɩ, na wɩrɛ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛ, na wɩrɛ a kɔɔ hanɩ jɔfʋ, na Thãgba fʋɔr bʋɔ, na wɩrɛ Thãgbaa ʋlfɛsɔ telenɩ,
45009005	kɛ dɔnɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩnaa məlsɔ. Kirisitii tibil dora wɛrra a the, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ kəəneni thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra gɩrɛ, Thãgba gɩ a hɩ̃ khɩɩrɛ waa khorr. Amɛn.
45009006	Sɩ ga do Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ debire a do mɔlɔ thɩ̃a', gɩdonɩ ga do wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛlɩ məl dʋɔn Ɩjɩrayɛldara ga.
45009007	Dɩ ga do wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ Abɩrahamɩ məl dʋɔn Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔa'. Sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ sor Abɩrahamna ayɩ: “Ɩjakɩɩ bɩsãsɔ wɛr na dɔ afɩ məl.”
45009008	Kɩrʋ dʋɔn, ga do bιsanaakɛ wι-n kɔnι wɛɛ kha wɛr n dɔ Thãgbaa bιsãsɔa'; sι ɔɔ məl dɔ bιsanaakɛ wι kɔnι mɔ̃ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnι ga har.
45009009	Hιnɛ gιrɛ dɔnι ʋlfɛ thιmιιrra gι sor ayι: “Wa bɔ caraakɛra ma birni ma-n ɩ̃ Sara na kʋɔn kũubir.”
45009010	Sι ga do gιrɛ dιbara ga, sι Rebekaa bιsãsɔ thι bιɛlι bisɔ wɛ, kɛ dɔnι Ɩjakι asι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃.
45009011	Gɩdonɩ bɩsanaale na thenɩ dɩɩra pɩ a na eʋʋ bɔɔ dɩ puure ga,
45009012	Thãgba kɔɔ sor Rebekara ayɩ: “Diine na dɔ kɔ̃tɩn cacadaarra.” Dι thɩ̃ɛ thakɛ daan gι nιna dι Thãgba n phire ʋrɛ a-n ƴaalnι dι wιι, sι ga do tibili thɩ̃ cʋʋra gι tha'.
45009013	Dι gι har mɔ̃ gι kherenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Jakɔbι mι na sa bo Ejayʋ.”
45009014	Dι mɔ̃ sa so gιrɛ? Thãgba na-n cʋʋ gιrɛɛkɛ telenenaa yaa? Kpιιraka'.
45009015	Gιdonι a sor Mʋιjιra ayι: “Ʋrɛ mι-n ƴaalnι ɩ̃ jι bʋɔra, mι-n jιιrɛ bʋɔra, dι ʋrɛ mι-n ƴaalnι bʋɔ n fɔ mι ɔrra, bʋɔ n fʋ mɛr ɔrra.”
45009016	Dι gɛr gι ga do gele ther ʋrɛraakɛ n ƴaalɛnιι pa, agιbo ʋrɛraakɛ na cʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛɛ pa ga, sι gι ther Thãgbaraakɛ n jιɛnnι tibil bʋɔra.
45009017	Gι sor Thãgbaa sɛbɛra aa, Thãgba sor Eaarɔna ayι: “Mɛr ιrɛ fι mɛna fι do nɔɔ ɩ̃ nιna ɩ̃ fãga, gι do nɔɔ dakha ɩ̃ i n kpaar thιιraakɛ koo.”
45009018	Gɛr gι a-n jιrɛ ʋrɛ a-n ƴaalnι a jι bʋɔra, sι dι cʋʋ ʋrɛ a-n ƴaalnɩ dɩ ɔɔda n khɩɩr.
45009019	Dɩ anaa fa bule mer: Dɩ a thale gɩ, anye Thãgba hana na so tibilidara, gɩdonɩ ʋmɔ̃ hale na lã gɩrɛraakɛ a-n ƴaalnɩ?
45009020	Ɩ̃ kuun, amɛ fɛrkɛ do a na banana Thãgba thɩ̃ banaa? Bʋlaakɛ wɩ-n mɩnɩ na bulele ʋrɛ n mɩɛnɩ, anyera a-n cʋʋ nι thalera ya?
45009021	Ga do mιmι n dɔ kɔ̃tιn jaarra gaa? Ja bulo bιɛlla a-n gba dι mιna bʋlaa yenyɔ, bιɛl n do bʋla ɓʋ̃ɔ, dι bιɛl n do thɔ̃ pɔι cʋʋdaa.
45009022	Dι ga do gιrɛ Thãgba cʋʋnι thalera gι ha gaa? A kɔɔ ƴaalɛ wer a nιnana ɔɔ nĩkhi a cʋʋna tɩbɩla wɩ jɩ mɔ̃ ɔɔ fãga hanɩ, sɩɩ do a fʋrɛ haar jɔɔ bʋlaasɔraakɛ teananɩ a ɩrɛna gar ɔɔ nĩkhirə, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ dananɩ kʋɛrɛ.
45009023	A kɔɔ ƴaalɛ dakha a nɩna bʋlaasɔɔkɛ a jɩnɩ bʋɔra mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ i dʋbɩrɔnɩ a thʋ̃ kãasɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ bʋlaasɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ maanɩ thɩɩnɛ gɩ 'lɛ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ;
45009024	dɩ sɛr wɛ, kɛ a kɔɔ wenɩ sɩ ga do Juifi caarra ɩkha the dɩbara ga, sɩ ca kpal ɩkha harrɛ.
45009025	Gɛr dʋɔn gɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ sonɩ Ojee sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Wɩrɛɛkɛ na kɔɔ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ toa', ma we wer ɩ̃ too. Dɩ ʋrɛ na kɔɔ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ nadaara', ma wɩɩrɛ ʋrɛ mɩ nanɩ.
45009026	Dɩ pa dɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ so warnɩ ayɩ: Na do ɩ̃ toa', liir wa we wɩ Thãgba yidaarɩ bikuunsɔ.”
45009027	Ejaɩ dakha hulene Ɩjɩrayɛldara ayɩ: “Adorakɛ Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsana jɔr a ho lanyɔ̃ gbalãkothɩn, sɩ gbe dɩbara na 'lɛ taarɛ;
45009028	gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ sonɩ, koo a na cʋʋ gɩ dɩ ga dã kɔrɔ thɩɩraakɛ.”
45009029	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ Ejaɩ kɔɔ 'laanɩ yɩɛ a sor ayɩ: “Ado Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ fãga koo hɩ̃daar na kɔɔ sɩ sar məl ɩkha gbə', sa kɔɔ honanɛna Sɔdɔm dɩɩ, sa kɔɔ horra Gɔmɔɔr dɩɩ.”
45009030	Dɩ mɔ̃ sa so gɩrɛ? Ca kpalaakɛ na-n kɔɔ dɔnɩ bʋɔ sor n hɛla war Thãgbaa ƴɛra ga, wɩ 'lɛr so hɛllɛ, sɩ so hɛllɛ gɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ ha pɛrɛra;
45009031	sɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldara wer kɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ so hɛl jɔfʋ, wa kɔɔ yɩ jɔfʋ thala'.
45009032	Mɔ̃ dɔ kɩrʋ? Gɩdonɩ ga do ha pɛrɛra wɩ kɔɔ ƴaal ga, sɩ awɩ thɔ̃ cʋʋra wɩ kɔɔ ƴaal gɩ. Nɛ bara bokaarra wɩ kɔɔ be nɔɔ,
45009033	dɩ gɩ har mɔ̃kɛra gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Hɩnɛ mɩ thɩɩnɛ nɛ bara bokaar Sɩyɔna, nɛ bara gbãgbaan gɩ, dɩ ʋrɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar ɔrra, ga ɩ̃ kpɩɩrakɛ a na dʋʋraa yicuruə'.”
45010001	Ɩ̃ omisɔ gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ na haar fɛʋ na gɩrɛ mɩ-n bɩɛllɔnɩ Thãgba dʋɔn ɩ̃ ca n 'lɛ taarɛ.
45010002	Mɩ jɩrɛ tue awɩdara dɩ wɩ hananɛ gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛ wer Thãgbaadara, sɩ wa hana jɩɩrɩkɛ teanana'.
45010003	Wa jɩnɩ kɩrʋ mɔ̃ Thãgba n hɛlnɩ tɩbɩlala sora', wɩ-n ƴaalɛ gɩ dɔ awɩ thɛthɛɛ bɔ dora sor hɛl war, dɩɩ do mɛ̃ wɩ bo so hɛllɛɛkɛ n thɛnɩ Thãgbara.
45010004	Gɩdonɩ Kirisitii pa liir jɔfʋ khu, dɩ mɛ̃ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haar na 'lɛ so hɛllɛ.
45010005	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ kherenɩ mɔ̃kɛ sor na hɛlnɩ tibillə jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛna ayɩ: “Tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ a na hana garɛ yire.”
45010006	Sɩ so hɛllɛɛkɛ n thɛnɩ ha pɛrɛra sor ayɩ: Fa-n so afɩ hara “amɛ na jʋnɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔa'“, a thɩɛna gaa gɩ cʋʋ Kirisiti a gbũ;
45010007	dɩ agɩbo “amɛ na gbuno tɩɛr dɩɩra ga”, a thɩɛna gaa gɩ cʋʋ Kirisiti a ɩɩr a the khirera.
45010008	Dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ so? Gɩ sor: “Thɩmɩɩrra na hʋnɔna fa', nɔɔ gɩ ha fɩ na haarra”, dɩ ha pɛ thɩmɩɩr gɩɩkɛ sɩ-n mɩɩnɩ.
45010009	Ado fɩ cã na afɩ nɔ ayɩ: Jeju dʋɔn Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ ado fɩ pɛr haar na afɩ bɩ̃ dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ ɩɩr a the khirera, fa 'lɛr taarɛ.
45010010	Gɩdonɩ ha pɛrɛ Jejura na bɩnɛ tibil n 'lɛrɔ so hɛllɛ, sɩ caan na nʋɔ tibil n 'lɛrɔ taarɛ.
45010011	Gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛhɛra ayɩ: “Tibil wo tibilikɛ pιɛrnι haar ɔrra, ga ɩ̃ kpιιrakɛ a na dʋʋraa yicuruə'.”
45010012	Dι Juifi na ha kpιι, na wιrɛ na dɔnι Juifisɔa ha kpιa', wɛr fɛʋ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιɛlla wι hana, kɛ ɔɔ bɔna jɔɔ n danι wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n wιɛnι.
45010013	Gιdonι Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayι: “Tibil wo tibilikɛ na wɛnι Kɔ̃tιnι i a na 'lɛr taarɛ.”
45010014	Dι mɔ̃ wa fʋ sι na wιι agado haar wι kɔɔ pɛr ɔrra boa? Dɩ mɔ̃ wa fʋ sι na pɛr haar ʋrɛraakɛ wa kɔɔ nιnι ɔɔ thιmιa? Dι mɔ̃ wa fʋ sι na nι ɔɔda ado mιmιι na hala?
45010015	Dι mɔ̃ mιmιa na fʋ sι na hale agado wι thɔ̃ wɛra? Gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Wιrɛ n ιnanι na tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι, awι ɩ̃ n daarɛ ka.”
45010016	Sι ga do fɛʋ kɔɔ tuon tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιa'; Ejaιɩ thɛthɛrakɛ kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ ayɩ: “Kɔ̃tɩn, amɛ pɩɛr haar gɩrɛraakɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ?”
45010017	Mɛ̃ ha pɛrɛ n the gɩrɛraakɛ tibil n nɩnɩ, dɩ gɩrɛra tibil n nɩnɩ Kirisitii thɩmɩɩra gɩ the.
45010018	Dɩ mɩ-n bulele: Wa ba nɩa yaa? Ɔɔ, wɩ nɩɛrɛ kɛ, mee Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “Awɩ nɔ kpaarɛ thɩɩraakɛ fɛʋ, dɩ awɩ thɩmɩɩ jaal a dã thɩɩ khu pa.”
45010019	Mɩ bire ma-n bule wo: Ɩjɩrayɛldara na kɔɔ jaa yaa? Mʋɩjɩ dɔ cacadaarɩkɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ: “Ma cʋʋrɛ dι gbugi na fʋ nι caarraakɛ na dɔnι caara'; Caarιkɛ na jɛnι thɩ̃a', ma cʋʋrɛ nĩkhii dɩ ga fʋ nɩ wɛrra.”
45010020	Dɩ Ejaɩ 'larrakɛ ɓoɓo a so: “Wɩrɛ na kɔɔ hana mɩnɩ ƴaala', wɩ yɩ mɛr; mɩ kɔɔ nɩnanɛ dɩbara wɩrɛɛkɛ na-n kɔɔ buleneni thɩ̃ɛ ɩ̃dara ga.”
45010021	Sɩ Ɩjɩrayɛldaraadara wer, a sor ayɩ: “Dɩwɩlʋ koo mɩ-n kɔɔ 'laa nyɛ̃ɛ caarraakɛ dɔnɩ nũ nʋra wa-n gba ɩ̃da ga.”
45011001	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɩ-n bulele ayɩ: Thãgba bor ɔɔ too yaa? Kpɩɩraka', gɩdonɩ mɛrɛ dakha Ɩjɩrayɛldaar ha mɩ, Abɩrahamɩ məl mɩ do, a do Bɛ̃jamɛ̃ɛ ca.
45011002	Thãgba na bo ɔɔ tookɛ a kɔɔ maanɩ jɩɩra'. Na jɩ thɩmɩɩ gɩrɛ kherenenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra, ka Elɩ mɩɩnanɩ Thãgba da-n pɛ Ɩjɩrayɛldara soraa, ayɩ:
45011003	“Kɔ̃tɩn wɩ kʋʋrɛ afι bobonasɔ a tʋɔrna afι bonι ji pasɔ a kpɛɛ, sιι do mɛr bιɛl sɛ gιrɛ 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ dι wι-n ƴaalɛ dakha ɩ̃ yʋ.”
45011004	Sι anye Thãgba sʋʋraa? “Mι tire kona gbιlanι makonyɔ wι dɔ ɩ̃da, kɛ na gulẽganɛnι a fʋɔr Baala'.”
45011005	Mɛna gι ha dakha nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ, wɛ hale sɛnι gbe kɛ Thãgba phiirni ɔɔ bɔ jιra.
45011006	Dι ado bɔ jιιrra gι, ga the thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra bã; ado thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra gι the, ga dor bɔ jιιr na do bɔ jιιr bã.
45011007	Dι mɔ̃ ga ha dɩphã? Gɩrɛ Ɩjɩrayɛldara n ƴaalnɩ wa kɔɔ 'lɛ ga, sɩ wɩrɛ Thãgba phiirni wer kɔɔ 'lɛ gɛr; sɩ wɩrɛ sɛnɩ awɩ ha dibire.
45011008	Dɩ gɩ har mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Thãgba kɔɔ hana wɩ haar thirfirii, na yinəəkɛ na dɔnɩ ga yɩra', na nũukɛ na dɔnɩ ga nɩra', a dana nĩkɛ.”
45011009	Dɩ Davɩdɩ sor ayɩ: “Awɩ dɩko kho pa n dɔ war waya na pheru, na ji paar, na so heeneekɛ na teana wɩnɩ.
45011010	Awɩ yi n hana thũu wa ya', dɩ cʋɛ wɩ wa-n gũguun wire koo.”
45011011	Dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ bule ayɩ: Nɔɔra Juifisɔ benɩ a ji, khorr wɩ ba ji yaa? Kpɩɩa'. Awɩ jirə dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ca kpala 'lɛ taarɛ gɩ cʋʋ gbugi gɩ fʋ wɛr Juifisɔ awɩdara.
45011012	Dɩ ado awɩ ji dor tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩraa bɔna 'lɛ pa, dɩ ado awɩ dɩ pa dor ca kpalaa bɔna 'lɛ pa, mɔ̃ awɩ nɔ dã na thʋ̃ na ha?
45011013	Sɩ nɛr ca kpala mɩ-n so gɩrɛ: Gɩdonɩ mɩ dor thɔ̃thɔn ca kpalala, mɩ-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛ ɩ̃ thɔna,
45011014	anaa ma yɩrɔrɛ fʋ paar ɩ̃ cʋʋ ɩ̃ ca gbugi n fʋ wɩ, ɩkhasɔ wɛrra n puno wɩ 'lɛ taarɛ.
45011015	Gɩdonɩ ado borɩkɛ Thãgba bo wɩnɩ dor tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ bir kũu kha na Thãgba, mɔ̃ awɩ bir gba na cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ na pɔna, ga dor khe birə a 'lɛ yirəə?
45011016	A wɩ ha Thãgba caca mɩ̃ bolookɛ wɩ khenɩ, koo dɔ daphuu, dɩ a thɩr nɛɛ do daphuu mɛ̃ jɛ̃ɛ na ha dakha.
45011017	Sɩ ado Thãgba kɔɔ kurre ɩkhaa olɩvɩ thɩr jɛ̃sɔ a faa sɩɩ do fɛrkɛ dɔnɩ hɔ̃ olɩvɩ thɩrʋ a gba fɛr a cooro, dɩɩ do ɔɔ nɛ na ɔɔ ƴɔ̃ fɩ bullo,
45011018	fa-n məbi jɛɛnaala'; sɩ ado fa məbi jɛ gɩ do ga do fɛr fʋɔn nɛa', sɩ nɛɛ fɔ fɩ jɩɩlna.
45011019	Sɩ fa sor nayɩ: Mee, jɛ̃ɛle kurre a faa sɩ ɩ̃ fi ɩ̃ cooro.
45011020	Sobɔr gɩ wer, gɩ kɔɔ kuurre a faa gɩdonɩ ga hana ha pɛra', sɩ fɛrɛ ha pɛrɛɛkɛ fɩ hananɩ gɛr dʋɔn afɩ too. Fa-n ti gunə', sɩ dɔ maar n ka fʋ fɩ.
45011021	Gɩdonɩ ado Thãgba na kɔɔ sɩ thɩr thernaa jɛna ga, a na sι far dakha ga.
45011022	Yɛ mɔ̃ Thãgba bɔrnι na wo mɔ̃ ɔɔda na-n wurnə': Wιrɛraakɛ jenι a-n nιna wɛr mɔ̃ ɔɔda na-n wurnə', sι fɛrɛra wer a-n nιna fɛr mɔ̃ a bɔrnι adora fι jιɛ too bɔɔbɔɔ ga bɔ caraalera, agado mɛ̃ ga fɛrɛ dakha a na kur fer na faa.
45011023	Wɛr Juifisɔ dakha wer, ado wa bo too awι baalla ga, Thãgba na coor wer kãkɛ wι kɔɔ hanι, gιdonι Thãgba hananɛ punone a na cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛ thale.
45011024	Ado nɛr ca kpalaakɛ dɔnι hɔ̃ olιvι thιr jɛ̃ɛ, kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ kurni a coor olιvι thιr thernanɛna sιι dorakɛ ga teena gι hana mã', mɔ̃ ga fʋ sιι do Juifisɔɔkɛ gbonι do olιvι thιr thernanɛ Thãgba na coor wι awι thɛthɛɛ olιvι thιrra ga?
45011025	Gɩdonɩ ma-n ƴaal nɩ omɩna na-n jɩ thɩ̃ gbulikaa ga, gɩ do nɔɔ na-n kpɩɛr waa gɩ ho thɩ̃ jɩna hana'; a thɩɛna gaa ga do Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa yaarra ƴɛrr ga jala', sɩ bɔɔkɛ ca kpala fɛʋ lonɩ na pɩ, dɩ nʋɔ dã, gɛr ga khuro;
45011026	mɛ̃ Ɩjɩrayɛl ɓibi na 'lɛ taarɛ, gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Sɩyɔna Taadaar na the, a na tire Jakɔbɩɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn thɩ̃ gõgolõ;
45011027	gɛr na dɔ ɩ̃ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ na wɛr, ɔbɔɔkɛ ma faanɩ awɩ sopugosɔ.”
45011028	Ado tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra gɩ, sobɔr gɩ wer, Juifisɔ dor lãlara na Thãgba, sɩ dɩ nɩ fi a ka yɩrɔ bɔɔ; sɩ ado phiirera gɩ, Thãgba na wɛr dɩɩ do awɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ dɔ nɔɔ.
45011029	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba na do dadebinaa ɔɔ khaarda 'laara na ɔɔ wera ga.
45011030	Mamara nɩ kɔɔ nʋʋrɛ nũu Thãgbara, sɩ nɛnɛ̃ Thãgba jɩ nɛr bʋɔra dɩɩ do Juifisɔɔ nũ nʋʋr dɔ nɔɔ.
45011031	Mɛna dakha Juifisɔ nʋʋr nũu nɛnɛ̃ gɩ do nɔɔ bʋɔraakɛ Thãgba jɩ nɩnɩ wɩ 'lɛrɔ dakha bɔ jɩɩr wer.
45011032	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba tor tɩbɩla fɛʋ nũ nʋʋrɛra gɩ do nɔɔ a jɩ wɩ fɛʋ bʋɔra.
45011033	Nɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ Thãgbaa dakpɛ do hanɩ, na mɔ̃ ɔɔ kpɛsɛ na ɔɔ jɩ huloni ɓoɓo. Ɔɔ kpɩɛr na ha 'lʋʋrra ga; ɔɔ fιlιkɛ a-n cʋʋnanι thɩ̃ɛ na ha jιιrra ga, mɔ̃kɛ gι kherenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι:
45011034	“Amɛ hale a jι Kɔ̃tιnι kpιɛr? Dι amɛ dɔ ɔɔ fιl dιιrdaar?
45011035	Amɛ dɔ cacadaar a kɔɔ ha Thãgba thɩ̃ɛ, dι na 'lar sι na bir na lιmʋʋ?”
45011036	Gɩdonɩ ɔr kɔɔ te thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, ɔr fʋɔn thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ jɩɩlna, dɩ ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ hale gɩrɛ. Ɔɔ i n dʋbarɔ na jala waa khorr. Amɛn.
45012001	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ jɔrnɩ ka, mɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr omɩna dɩ na gba anɩ dɩbara a na ha Thãgba, gɩ do bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hananɩ yire, a do daphuu, a da Thãgba haar, gɛr dɔ fʋɔr bʋɔɔkɛ na-n fʋɔrʋʋnɩ.
45012002	Na-n hana ga fɩlɩkɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩra hananɩ gɩra', sɩ nɩ dɔ Thãgba n debi anɩ kpɩɛrsɔ koo gɩ do nɔɔ nɩ hana ha phaa, liir na puno dɩphã na-n jɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ dɩɩ daaraa haar, ga hana dakha dɩ paara'.
45012003	Khaardaakɛ Thãgba ha mɩnɩ ɔɔ bɔ jɩra, gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma-n so nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛlla, dɩ na-n hana dɩbara khəi kpɩɛrɛ gɩ jɔ gɩrɛ mɩɛna nɩna', sɩ nɩ dɔ gɩ do kpɩɛrɛɛkɛ mɩɛna nɩnɩ, gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ ha pɛrɛɛkɛ Thãgba ha nɩnɩ bɩɛlbɩɛl hanɩ.
45012004	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ hananɩ tomɩ ɓanasɔ dɩɩdɩɩ tomɩ bɩɛlla, sɩɩ do tomɩ ɓãasɔra na hana thɔ̃ bɩɛla';
45012005	mɛ̃ gɩ ha na sɛrɛ, sɩ jɔrnɩɩkɛrakɛ sɩ tomɩ bɩɛl sɩ do dɩɩ the asɩ bɩɛl dora nakha Kirisiti, dɩ sɛrɛ fɛʋ coore kha ʋ do ʋʋ tomɩ ɓã, dɩ ʋ do ʋʋ tomɩ ɓã.
45012006	Sɩ mɔ̃ sɩ hananɩ khaardaasɔ fɛʋ dɩɩdɩɩ mɔ̃kɛ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ Thãgba jɩ sɩnɩ hanɩ, ado ntɛɛ khaarda dʋɔn Thãgba tukɩr tir, a na-n mɩa ga-n mɩɛna ha pɛrɛɛkɛ a hananɩ.
45012007	Ado bubul thɔma gɩ, ntɛ na-n jalana gɩ; a tibil dɩɩrɛ gɩ, ntɛ na-n jalana gɩ;
45012008	ado yɩr thɩmɩɩr ntɛ hana a na-n jalana gɩ, ʋrɛ n 'laanɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ, a na-n 'laanɛ na bɩ̃ bʋɔ; ʋrɛ 'lɛnɩ ƴɛ kʋʋlɛ, a na-n tɛrɔ ɔɔ thɔnana; ʋrɛ hananɩ bɔ jɩɩr, a na-n jɛ bʋɔrara na daʋ.
45012009	Na-n do dι anι naʋ na-n hana fιιla'; na-n ƴʋɔnɛ thɩ̃ puu sa ma thɩ̃ bʋɔra kĩkĩkĩ.
45012010	Ado omi naarra gι, na-n na kha na naʋʋkɛ hanι phãphãphã; kɔɔ kʋlɛ ƴιɛ a na cɔ haan ga-n hulono.
45012011	Ado thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra gι na-n hana dokhʋʋra'; nι hana phãphãphã haarra; na-n dɔ Kɔ̃tιnι thɔ̃.
45012012	Nι dɔ nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ nι hananι n cʋʋ nι na-n kãka; na-n fɔ haar bɔ gaarɛra; na-n yιra Thãgba bιɛlɛla;
45012013	ha pɛdaraakɛ thɩ̃ɛ n ɓɔrnι na-n bulo wi; na-n bãbanɛ na kpakpal teere.
45012014	Na-n bɔna wιrɛ n kpoone narnι, na-n bɔna wι na-n yι sʋɔn n 'le wa'.
45012015	Na-n kãkanɛ na wιrɛ n kãkanɛnι, sι na-n bɛ na wɩrɛ n bιɛnnι.
45012016	Na-n hιnɛ khasɔ bιɛlbιɛl na fιl bιɛl. Na-n ka kʋʋra', sι na-n hana kha na wιrɛɛkɛ tιbιla na-n thernana'. Na-n hιιn anιbara mɔ̃ nι donι tιι kpɛsɛsɔa'.
45012017	A tibil cʋʋ nɩ puure na-n bir cʋgʋʋ puurə'. Na-n ƴaalɛ gιrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra.
45012018	A nι yι hʋɛ, nι dɔ bʋɔ na tɔɔ kha na ha ιι na tιbιla fɛʋ.
45012019	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mι-n nanι na-n tiir helua', sι nι sɛrɔ Thãgbaa nĩkhi a tiir. Gιdonι Kɔ̃tιn sor Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Hel tiire dɔ ιda, dι mɛr dɔ ʋrɛ na lιmanι tibil gιrɛ a cʋʋnɩ.”
45012020	Sɩ “a kɔmɛr fʋ afɩ lãlaardaar hanaa dɩkor, a yɔlkhaa fʋʋ hanaa nyʋɔn; gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ fɩ-n cʋʋnɩ thale ga dor nɔɔ, yicuruukɛ hɔnɩ dɔɔ n fʋʋ.”
45012021	Fa-n do puure na-n puno fa', sɩ dɔ fɩ ka fɩ kəə puurera ga-n the afɩ bɔ cʋʋra.
45013001	Dɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na-n nɩ nũu wɩrɛraakɛ dɔ warnɩ fãgadara, gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ yʋʋ na hale saagado Thãgba pɛ waraa ga, dɩ fãgadaraakɛ hanɩkɛ nɛnɛ̃kɛ Thãgba pɛ war.
45013002	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n lananɩ wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ yʋʋ, jɔfʋʋkɛ Thãgba pɛrnɩ a-n laan, dɩ wɩrɛ n lananɩ wa gbaar sor na heen dɩbara.
45013003	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ bɔɔ fãga hɩ̃dara na-n kʋ wɩ maara', sɩ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ puure, wɛr wɩ-n kʋ maar. A fa ƴaal wɩrɛ dɔ farnɩ yʋʋ na-n kɔ fɩ maara', na cʋɛ bɔɔ fa yɩ gɛr dɩ wa khɩɩ fɩ.
45013004	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃daar a do thɩ̃ɛ na-n bɔ far; sɩ ado fa cʋʋ puure wer, dɔ maar na-n fʋ fɩ gɩdonɩ ga do mɔlɔ a-n fʋrɔ bajɩna ga, sɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃daar a do hel tiirera, a na-n nɩnana puu cʋʋdara ɔɔ nĩkhi.
45013005	Dɩ gɛr gɩ gɩ teenanɛ fa-n nɩ nũu, ga do nĩkhiirəəle dɔ nɔɔ dɩbara ga, sɩ gɩdonɩ fɩ yɩ gɛr le haarra dɩɩ do gɛr bʋɔnɔ.
45013006	Gelela dɔ nɔɔ dakha dɩ na-n lɩmɩnɔ lãpho, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃dara fãgadara do, kɛ n dɔnɩ ga thɔ̃ caalera bɔɔbɔɔ.
45013007	Na-n hana tɩbɩla fɛʋ gɩrɛ ntɛ teenanɩ: Ʋrɛ n gbaannɩ lãpho, na-n lɩmaa ɔɔ lãpho; gɩrɛ dʋɔnyɛ̃ n buleni, na-n lɩma; ʋrɛ teananɩ maar na-n maanɛɛ; ʋrɛ teananɩ cʋʋr na-n cʋɔnɛɛ.
45013008	Na-n hana tibil bɩɛl helua'; heluukɛ dɩbara teananɩ nɩ hanana dʋɔn naʋʋkɛ na-n nanɩ kha; gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ naannɩ ɔɔ 'walãkha tibil, a cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛ fɛʋ jɔfʋ n ƴaalnɩ ga-n cʋɛ.
45013009	Gɩdonɩ jɔfʋʋkɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ: “Fa-n hana khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n hana kũu kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n kʋ tibilə', fa-n yuə', fa-n pɩɛr hara ga”, na gɩ̃j ɔfʋ kpɩɩ fɛʋ, thɩmɩɩ nɔ bɩɛlla gɩ gbɛbɩ do ayɩ: “Fa-n na afɩ 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃kɛ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara.”
45013010	Naʋ na-n cʋʋ ɔɔ 'walãkha tibil puurə', dɩ gɛr gɩ ado naʋ hale ga dor jɔfʋ koo cʋʋrɛ a dã.
45013011	Dι mɔna nɩ-n cʋʋnɩ mɛna, nɩ jɛna gɩ dɩ bɔɔ daan, dɩ bɔɔ gɩɩkɛ teananɩ nɩ jaa daanɔ mɛ̃, gɩdonɩ nɛnɛ̃ taarɛ wɔrɔ̃ sɛr a jɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ pɛrnɩ haar.
45013012	Dɩɩ tɩnɛ dɩ ga-n thɔɔ wɩllɛ, dɩɩ do dɩwɩlʋ wɔrɔnɛ mɛ̃; sɩ dɔna dabirəə thɔ̃ a faa, sa tɔ ko ke thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ dahɩrɛɛda.
45013013	Sa-n ɩrɛ na fɩl telẽe gɩ ho nɩɔ̃kɛ tibil na-n ɩɩrnɩ dɩwɩlʋla. Sa-n ɩɩrna gbõgolõ dɩko khor na ta laara', na khɛ laarɛ na kũu laara', na dakhaba cʋʋra', na-n ɩɩrna kɩla na gbugə'.
45013014	Sɩ nɩ gba Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn a tɔ; na-n ƴaal nɩ cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ ga-n da anɩ tibil do paraakɛ thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛ n kʋnɩ thueə'.
45014001	Nɩ tea ʋrɛ na tɩɛnnɩ ha pɛrɛra ga, sɩ na-n bana kha kpɩɛr hananɛnasɔ dɩɩdɩa'.
45014002	Ʋ na hananɛ ha pɛrɛ a na-n kho thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, sɩ ʋrɛ na tɩɛnnɩ ha pɛrɛra ga, ga dor fa haar or na-n kho.
45014003	Ʋrɛ n khɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ a na-n beesi ʋrɛ na-n khɔnaa ga; dɩ ʋrɛ n khɔnɩ fa haar a na-n 'laa na yɩ dɩɩ ʋrɛraakɛ n khɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋa', gɩdonɩ Thãgba teaa.
45014004	Amɛ fɛrkɛ do dɩ fa-n kɩɩlna haanɩ thɔ̃daar? Ado a jɩɩlɛ, ado a jire, ɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ gɩ ba, sɩ a na jɩɩlɛ gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩn hananɛ punone a na fʋnaa.
45014005	Ʋkha n tirore wi bɩɛl dɩɩ dʋʋraa wi kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ a jɔ gɩ̃ wi fɛʋ, sɩ ʋ na-n hɩɩnɛ wiresɔ gɩ dʋʋraa bɩɛl. Dɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl n jɩɩ jɩ tue bɔɔbɔɔ awɩ hara ga kpɩɛrraale.
45014006	Ʋrɛ n teronɩ wire dɩɩ ha kpɩɩ, a tirore ga-n cɔ Kɔ̃tɩn; ʋrɛ n khɔnɩ a-n khor ga-n cɔ Kɔ̃tɩn, gɩdonɩ Thãgba a-n fʋɔr sɩ da-n kho; sɩ ʋrɛ n bɔnɩ khor, a-n bor ga-n cɔ Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ ɔrra dakha Thãgbara a-n fʋɔr.
45014007	Gɩdonɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na-n hana yire dɩɩ do ɔɔ thɛthɛɛda dɩbara ga, dɩ tibil na-n khi dɩɩ do ɔɔ thɛthɛɛda dɩbara ga.
45014008	Gɩdonɩ a sɩ hana yire, sɩ hana gɛr dɩɩ do Kɔ̃tɩnɩda, dɩ a sɩ khire Kɔ̃tɩnɩdara gɩ do; dɩ gɛr gɩ a yire sɩ hana, a sɩ khire yo, sɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩdara sɩ do.
45014009	Gɛr hɩna dɩ Kirisiti kɔɔ khi sa bir ɩɩr a the khirera dɩ mɛ̃ a na do Kɔ̃tɩn khĩdidarara na yidarara.
45014010	Sɩ fɛrɛ, mɔ̃ dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ fa-n kɩɩlna afɩ omi? Dɩ fɛrɛ wo, anyera fɩ-n beesi afɩ omi? Mee sɛrɛ fɛʋ sa jaal na jɩɩl Thãgbara kɩɩl paar.
45014011	Gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Mɔ̃kɛ mɩ donɩ yidaar mɛ̃ ga ha, mɛr Kɔ̃tɩn sɔ, nɛkhilə ɓibi na gulẽga marɛ, dɩ delẽbe ɓibi na caan ɩ̃ Thãgba do.”
45014012	Mɛ̃ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl na mɩɩna Thãgba mɔ̃ awɩ thɛthɛɛda hanɩ.
45014013	Gɛr gι sa-n 'laa na yι kha dιι bιɛlbιɛl bã, sι asι ƴaal n ka dɔ sa-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ gι cʋʋ asι omi a bara a jə'.
45014014	Mɔ̃ mι donι Jeju Kɔ̃tιnιda, mι jι gɛr a jιna tue dι thɩ̃ bιɛllakɛ na hale dɔnɩ dasãsιnaa ga; sι ado tibil na hιιn thɩ̃ doo nɩɔ̃ gɩ don donɩ thĩ sãsɩnaa, thɩ̃ sãsιnaana ga dʋʋraa ger.
45014015	Ado gιrɛ fι-n khonɩ pɛr afɩ omina kpɩɛr nyanyaanɛ, ga do naʋ fɩ-n jalna bã. Fa-n do afɩ dakhona n cʋʋ ʋrɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ khironi a buə'.
45014016	Na-n do gɩrɛ dɔ narnɩ dabʋɔ n do nɔɔ tɩbɩla na-n mɩɩrɔ dapuə'.
45014017	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do, ga do dɩko thɩmɩɩr gɩ na thɩ̃ yɔnana', sɩ fɩl sarʋ, na ha ɩɩ, na daʋ gɩ do, dɩɩ the Thu Phuurə.
45014018	Ʋrɛ n dɔnɩ Kirisitii thɔ̃ na ga fɩl caale, ɔr n da Thãgba haar, dɩ tɩbɩla n khɩsʋʋrɛ dakha.
45014019	Gɛr gι sa-n ƴaalɛ gιrɛ na 'laanɛnι ha ιι, na gιrɛ na cʋɛnι ʋ a khɔ̃ a na-n pɛr ʋ n khɔ̃ a na-n pɛr.
45014020	Fa-n kʋɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃ dιko pιɛrʋʋra ga. Sobɔr gι wer thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ phure, sι gι puurore tibillə ado a na kho dιι debi a do nɛ bara bokaar.
45014021	Gι bɔrɛ dι fa bo nʋʋn, na bona taan, na bona gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na cʋɛnι afι omi dι na bara, agιbo a ji, agιbo gι dʋʋraa yɔɔ paar.
45014022	Ha pɛ ca ole fι hananι gelela, fɔrɔ gι do afιda fɛrɛ na Thãgba. Gι-n dar tibilləəkɛ hananι tu jιιr thιɛnaakɛ a pɛrnι haar, sι ga-n bir dιι dʋʋraa so heene haarra ga.
45014023	Sɩ ʋrɛ hananɩ baalɛ gɩrɛraakɛ a-n khonɩ sor n heenuune, gɩdonɩ ɔɔ eʋʋ pa na the ha pɛrɛra ga. Dɩ mee gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na thɛnι ha pɛrɛra ga, sopugo gι.
45015001	Sɛrɛɛkɛ tιɛnnι ha pɛrɛra sι teenanɛ sa-n bulo wιrɛ na tιɛnnι ha pɛrɛra ga, sι sa-n kpιɛrna gιrɛ na dãa sarna'.
45015002	Dɔ sɛrɛ fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl na-n cʋʋ gɩrɛ na danɩ asɩ 'walãkha tibillə, kɛ na dʋɔraanɩ thɩ̃ bʋɔ, gɩ cʋʋ khɔ̃ pɛrɛ ga-n hale.
45015003	Gιdonι Kirisiti dakha na kɔɔ ƴaal gιrɛ daaraanι dιbara ga, sι gι har mɔ̃kɛ gι kherenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Nιιrɛɛkɛ nιnιra kɔɔ nιιr fιnι kɔɔ heen mer.”
45015004	Dι gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ kherenenι mamara gι kɔɔ kherere gι dιιr sι thɩ̃ɛ, dι ha fʋrɛ na ha faarɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ n 'laanι na dor nɔɔ dɩ sa hana nũ pɛrɛ.
45015005	Dɔ Thãgbaakɛ ha fʋrɛ na ha faarɛ n thernɩ n cʋʋ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl nɩ hana kpɩɛr bɩɛl, gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ Jeju Kirisitiida hanɩ;
45015006	dɩ mɛ̃ na hana kha bɩ̃ bɩɛl, na nɔ bɩɛl, na-n khɩɩna Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii Thɩ.
45015007	Dι gɛr gι na-n tea kha bιɛlbιɛl mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ tee nιnι gι cʋʋ Thãgbaa i gι dʋbιrɔ.
45015008	Gιdonι mι sor ayι: Kirisiti debire a do thɔ̃daar Juifisɔraakɛ n kuroni khʋ̃ʋ, gι nιna Thãgbaa sobɔdaar do, mɔ̃kɛ a-n cʋʋnι gιrɛ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanι asι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ,
45015009	ca kpala dakha na-n khɩɩ Thãgba ɔɔ bɔ donana, gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Gɛr gɩ dɩ ma khɩɩ fɩ ca kpalaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, afɩ i dʋbɩ nɩ ma khɩ̃.”
45015010	Dɩ gɩ sor wo ayɩ: “Ca kpala na-n kãkanɛ kha na ɔɔ too.”
45015011	Wo: “Nɛr ca kpala fɛʋ, na-n khɩa Kɔ̃tɩn; dɔ tibil caar fɛʋ na-n khɩsʋʋ.”
45015012	Wo Ejaɩ sor dakha ayɩ: “Ɩjaɩɩ məl ʋkha na ɩnɛ, a na ɩɩrɛ na gba fãga ca kpalala, dɩ ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ ca kpala na pɛrnɩ haar.”
45015013	Thãgbaakɛ nũ pɛrɛ n theronɩ n cʋɛ daʋ na ha ɩɩ fɛʋ gɩ hi anɩ hara, gɩ the anɩ ha pɛraakɛ nɩ hananɩ ɔrra, gɩ do nɔɔ Thu Phuu n cʋʋ nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ nɩ hananɩ ɔrra gɩ thʋ̃ gɩ kãasɩ.
45015014	Ado mɛr gɩ, ɩ̃ omisɔ, mɩ jɩrɛ tue gɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ anɩda, gɛr dʋɔn mɔ̃ nɩ hananɩ bɔ cʋʋrɛ ka, a hanana jιιr ɓibi, a hanana punone a na dιιrna khasɔ.
45015015	Sɩrakɛ ɩ̃ sɛbɛraakɛ mɩ khere narnɩ paarsɔ hale mɩ 'lanɩ a mɩɩ nɩ thɩ̃ɛ casɩ, gɩ cʋʋ nɩ nɩ hana jɩnanɛ thɩ̃ ɩkhara, dɩ mɩ kherere thakɛ dɩɩ the bɔ jɩɩrraakɛ Thãgba jɩ mɩnɩ bʋɔra,
45015016	dɩ ma do Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃daar ca kpalala; Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ gbõdaar thɔ̃ɔkɛ mɩ-n cʋʋnɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ ca kpala na ho bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ danɩ Thãgba haar, kɛ Thu Phuu leenɩ kpɩɩ dɩɩ do ɔɔda.
45015017	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɩ hananɛ gɩrɛ ma məbironi Thãgbaa ƴɛra dɩ gɩ ther ɩ̃ bɩɛl dora na Jeju Kirisiti.
45015018	Gɩdonɩ ma 'la na mɩɩ thɩ̃ kpɩa', sɩ gɩrɛ Kirisiti gba mɩnɩ da-n cʋʋna ca kpala na-n nɛ nũu gɩ, gɩ the ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩra, na ɩ̃ thɩ̃ cʋʋra,
45015019	na fãgaakɛ yɩranɩ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra, na ma kʋ thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra, na Thu Phuu fãgara; mɛ̃ mι kɔɔ fʋ Jerujalɛm a mιι Kirisitii tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιιra jɔɔ a finə a ba dana Iliri.
45015020	Dι gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ kɔɔ dʋɔn ma-n mɩa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ ka wa kɔɔ nɩnɩ Kirisitii i pa', dɩ mɛ̃ ma dɛbɩ tɩɩ kpɩɩ go kpɛɛra ga.
45015021	Sɩ gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Wɩrɛraakɛ ɔɔda na kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ kpɩɩa', wa yɩɩrɛ, dɩ wɩrɛ na kɔɔ nɩɛnɛna', wa jɩrɛ kɩrʋ.”
45015022	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ mɩnɩ bɔ jɔjʋɔra dɩ ma kɔɔ pɔ anɩ pa ga.
45015023	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ ma hana paarɩkɛ ma doronɩ thɔma bəənnəəkɛ bã; sɩɩ do yɛna jɔrɛ gɩrɛ mɩ kɔɔ ƴaalnɩ ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa,
45015024	ɔbɔɔkɛ ma-n kanɩ Esɩpanyɩ. Mɩ pɛrɛ haar ɩ̃ yɛ nɩ a ma ka, dɩ mɩ nar ɩ̃ tɔɔ ɓo gbe anɩ pa a he, sɩ nɩ thɔɔ mɩ.
45015025	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ Jerujalɛm mɩ-n jal gɩrɛ ɩ̃ bulnə tɩɩ phuusɔ.
45015026	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ hanɩ Masedʋan na Akaɩ gɩ kɔɔ da warɛ haar dɩ wɩ pɛ thɩ̃ɛ gɩ bul bɔdaraakɛ hanɩ tɩɩ phuusɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn Jerujalɛm.
45015027	Gɩ kɔɔ da warɛ haar bɔɔbɔɔ, dɩrakɛ thɩ̃ɛ gɩɩkɛ wɩ teenanɩ wɩ cʋɛ, gɩdonɩ ado wɛr ca kpala Juifisɔɔ pa wɩ 'lɛ thu thɩ̃ɛ, wɩ teenanɛ dakha wa-n bulo wi na nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ thɩ̃sɔ.
45015028	A mι 'li pιr ga thɔ̃ɔle a 'li gbaar khaardaale a dʋ wι nyɔ̃kɔɔ, gɛr ma jaal Esιpanyι, sι anι pa ma the sι na ka.
45015029	Mι jιrɛ ado ma pɔ anι pa Kirisitii bɔna ma pɔna nyɔ̃kor hire phi.
45015030	Omιna, asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii i na naʋʋkɛ Thu Phuu n 'laanι mι gba, dι ma-n phʋʋrna nι dι na kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ na-n ɓã mι anι Thãgba bιɛllaakɛ nι-n bιɛlnι dι na-n pɛ mar,
45015031	gι do nɔɔ a taa mι Jude ha pɛ 'leedaraa nyɔ̃kɔɔ, dι mɛ̃ dakha wo khaardaakɛ mι-n jalnanι gιrɛ Jerujalɛm tιι phuusɔ n tee gι na daʋ,
45015032	gι do nɔɔ, ado Thãgba tuur gι ɩ̃ dã anι pa na daʋ, ɩ̃ 'lɛ nar dakha hιιrɛ.
45015033	Thãgbaakɛ ha ιι n thernι n hana kha na nɛrɛ fɛʋ. Amɛn.
45016001	Mι-n ƴaalɛ nι jɛ dι asι õkhɛr Eəbeekɛ dɔnι Sãkιrɛ we gbɛbιdaraa thɔ̃ dodaar, tιι teena a do.
45016002	Nι teaa Kɔ̃tιnι tee na fιlɛɛkɛ tιι phuusɔ teenanι wι hanana. Nι tɔɔ ga too a na buloo thɩ̃ɛ wo thιɛnaakɛ a na hana narnι ƴaalɛ, gιdonι ɔr dakha a kɔɔ bulle tibil jɔjʋɔ ka na mɛrkɛrakɛ dakha.
45016003	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Pirisika na Akɩlasɩ wɛrkɛ sɩ-n donanɩ kha Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃.
45016004	Awɩ yi na kɔɔ burera ɩ̃ sora, sɩ ga do mɛr dɩbara n fʋɔrɛ wɩ gelela ga, sɩ we gbɛbɩdara fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ ca kpalaa thɩ̃thɩɩn fʋɔr wɛr ga sora.
45016005	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ dakha we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ n gbɛbanɩ kha awɩ cɔ. Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Epaɩnɛtɩɩkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, ɔr dɔ caca tibilikɛ pɛnɩ Kirisiti haar Ajɩ dɩɩra.
45016006	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Marɩɩkɛ dɔ marnɩ thɔma jɔɔ ka.
45016007	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Ãdʋrɔnɩkasɩ na Junɩasɩ wɛrkɛ dɔ marnɩ toona, kɛ sɩ cʋʋnanɩ kha khaɩ, kɛ thɛnɩ ire ka thɔ̃thɔnaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, kɛrakɛ kɔɔ kʋlɛ mɩnɩ ƴιɛ a pɛr Kirisiti haar.
45016008	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Ãpɩlɩasɩɩkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra.
45016009	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Ʋrbɛ̃ɛkɛ sɩ-n donanɩ kha Kirisitii thɔ̃, na Sɩtakɩsɩɩkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ.
45016010	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Apɛlɛsɩɩkɛ kɔɔ nɛnanɩ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ ha pɛ Kirisitira hanɩ. Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Arɩsɩtobulɩ cɔdara.
45016011	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Ɛrɔdɩyɔ̃ ɩ̃ tibil; nɩ fʋɔrɛ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda, kɛ dɔnɩ Narsɩsɩɩ cɔdara.
45016012	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Tɩrɩfɛn na Tɩrɩfosɩ wɛrkɛ n dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃ jɔɔ ka. Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Pɛrsɩɩdɩɩkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, kɛ kɔɔ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃ dɩɩ thʋ̃ kar.
45016013	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Rufusiikɛ teronɩ a ha kpɩɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃ dora, a fʋɔrna ɔɔ nɩɩkɛ dɔ marnɩ dakha nɩrɛ.
45016014	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Asɛ̃kɩrɩtɩ, na Filegɔ̃, na Ɛrmɛsɩ, na Paturobasɩ, na Ɛrmasɩ, na omɩnaakɛ wɩ hananɩ kha.
45016015	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ Filoloogi, na Juli, na Nere na ɔɔ õkhɛr, na Olɛ̃pɩ, na tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ hananɩ kha.
45016016	Na-n fʋɔrɛ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl na ha lõ fʋɔrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ daphuu. Kirisitii we gbɛbɩdara fɛʋ fʋɔr nɛr.
45016017	Mɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr omɩna dɩ na jɩɩ dʋ bʋrɛ wɩrɛraakɛ n pɩɛrnɩ leere na nɛ baradaa, dɩ wa-n kʋɛ dɩɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ; na-n jana wa tibil casɔraale.
45016018	Gɩdonɩ tibil ca wele ga do Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ thɔ̃ wɩ-n doa', sɩ gɩrɛ n danɩ awɩ tomɩra wɩ-n yɩrna; dɩ wɩ gba nɔ da thɩmɩa, na fɩɩlɛ, wa-n fɩɩlna tɩbɩlaakɛ na hananɩ jɩɩr bɔɔbɔa'.
45016019	Tɩbɩla fɛʋ nɩrɛ mɔ̃ anɩ nũ nɩ hanɩ, gɛr gɩ anɩda da marɛ kpɛ, sɩ mɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɩ hanana kpɛsɛrɛ a na jɛna thɩ̃ bʋɔ, sa dɔ yʋ 'leedara thɩ̃ puu cʋʋrɛra.
45016020	Kιɛr na gbe Thãgbaakɛ ha ιι n thernι na cʋɔrɛ Satãa yʋ anι nɛ ballɔ. Asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju na-n jɛ nι bʋɔra.
45016021	Timotheekɛ sι-n donanι kha thɔma fʋɔr nɛr; Lusiyusi na Jajɔ̃ na Sojɩpatɛɛr wɛrkɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ too wɩ fʋɔr nɛr.
45016022	Mɛr Tɛrtiyusiikɛ Pol pɛrnɩ dɩ ɩ̃ khere sɛbɛɛkɛ, mɩ fʋɔr nɛr mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tιnɩda.
45016023	Gayʋsɩɩkɛ tea mɩnɩ kpakpaalɛ, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛɛ pa we gbɛbɩdara n gbɛbɩnɩ kha, a fʋɔr nɛr. Erasɩtɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ war fʋrɔdaar dɩɩra, na asɩ omi Kartusi wɩ fʋɔr nɛr dakha.
45016024	[Asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra.]
45016025	Thãgba hιna khιιrɛ, ɔr gɩɩkɛ hananɩ punone a na cʋʋna nɩ dɩ na tɩ, gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ mɩ-n mɩɩnι hanι, kɛ n mιanι Jeju Kirisitiida, gι ha dakha mɔ̃ thɩ̃ gbulikɛ kɔɔ maanι kerre sa yιr dιphã hanι,
45016026	dι gι nιrɔrɛ nɛnɛ̃ casι, Thãgbaa bobonaa sɛbɛ mιa gι; dι Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι khorrdaar ɔr pιɛr tibil caar fɛʋ n jɛ gι, wι puno wι pɛr haar wa-n nι nũu.
45016027	Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι bιɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽekɛ hιnanι kpɛsɛrɛ, ɔr n hιna i dʋbιrɛ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ, gɩ do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ. Amɛn.
46001001	Mɛr Polɩkɛ Thãgba wenɩ dɩ ɩ̃ do Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni, na Sɔsɩtɛnɩkɛ dɔnɩ omine,
46001002	thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ hanɩ Korɛ̃tɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ leanɩ kpɩɩ a ha Jeju Kirisitira, kɛ Thãgba wenɩ dɩ wɩ do tibil phuusɔ mɔ̃kɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ paar wo paar, kɛ n fʋɔrɛnɩ Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ hanɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ awɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na asɩda.
46001003	Thãgba asɩ Thɩ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn n hana nɩ ha ɩɩ, a jɛ nɩ dakha bʋɔra.
46001004	Wire wo wire mɩ-n khɩɩ ɩ̃ Thãgba anɩ sora, mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ nɩnɩ bʋɔra dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
46001005	Gɩdonɩ ɔrra nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛ ler thɩɛna fɛʋ dɩɩdɩɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ, thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛ fɛʋ na jɩɩr fɛʋ,
46001006	dɩɩ the gɩrɛraakɛ sobɔ so jɩɩr Kirisitira kɔɔ tɩnɩ kɩbɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn;
46001007	dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgbaa khaarda bɩɛllakɛ na ɓɔr nɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ toonɩ gɩrɛ dɩ na-n pɩɛr asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii nɩrɔa'.
46001008	Ɔr na cʋɛ nɩ dakha dɩ na tɩ gɩ dana khu paar, dɩ mɛ̃ na hana so paar asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii wirə ga.
46001009	Sobɔdaar Thãgba do, ɔrkɛ kɔɔ wɛ nɩnɩ nɩ dɔ kha kũu bɩnɔ na ɔɔ Bikuun Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃.
46001010	Omɩna, asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii i mɩ gba dɩ ma-n phʋʋrna nɩ, dɔ na-n mɩɩ kha nɔ bɩɛl, na-n do leere n ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩna', sɩ nɩ fɔ kha bɔɔbɔɔ a hanana kpɩɛr bɩɛl na nɔ bɩɛl.
46001011	Gɩdonɩ ɩ̃ omisɔ mɩ nɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ anɩ pa dɩ Kʋloee too mɩɩ mɩ ayɩ, kɩla n har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
46001012	A thɩɛna gaa nɛrɛ bɩɛlbɩɛlɩ pa ʋ n yɩ, ine wer Polɩda ɩnɩ do; ʋ n yɩ, ine wer Apolɔsɩɩda ɩnɩ do; ʋ n yɩ, ine wer Sefasɩɩda ɩnɩ do; ʋ n yɩ, ine wer Kirisitiida ɩnɩ do.
46001013	Tɩnɛ paar kɔɔ har Kirisitira kã? Wɩ kɔɔ kpar Pol kʋkʋ thɩrʋra anɩ sora kã? Dɩ agɩbo Polɩ i dɔ gɩrɛ wɩ gbanɩ a kpɛɛna nɩ nyʋɔnɔ yaa?
46001014	Mɩ-n khɩɩrɛ Thãgba gɩrɛraakɛ ma kɔɔ kpɛɛnɩ tibil nɛrɛra nyʋɔnɔ saagado Kirisipusi na Gayʋsɩ gaaga;
46001015	dɩ mɛ̃ tibil na puno na so nayɩ ɩ̃ i wɩ kɔɔ gba a kpɛɛna nɩ nyʋɔnɔa'.
46001016	Wo Sɩtefanasɩɩ cɔdara mɩ kɔɔ kpɛɛ nyʋɔnɔ, sɩ ado ntɛ halerakɛ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ kpɛgʋʋ nyʋɔnɔ ma ja'.
46001017	Gɩdonɩ Kirisiti na kɔɔ thɔ̃ mɩ ma-n kpɛa tɩbɩla nyʋɔnɔa', sɩ ma-n mɩa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, sɩ ma-n gba thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ thɛnɩ tibil kpɛsɛra a na mɩɩna gɩ ho ga ba cʋʋrɛ Kirisitii kʋkʋ thιr gι debi gι do mɔlɔa'.
46001018	Gιdonι Kirisitii khi kʋkʋ thιrʋra, ga thιmιι dor də̃bəəle wιrɛraakɛ n buureni, sι ado sɛrra wɛ, kɛ 'lɛnι taarɛ, Thãgbaa fãga gι do sar.
46001019	Gιdonι gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Ma wιɛlɛ kpɛsɛdaraa kpɛsɛ, ma bũburone thɩ̃ jιnaa jι.”
46001020	Ka tɩɩ kpɛsɛ ha? Ka sɛbɛ kheredaar ha? Ka nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ thɩ̃ banadaar ha? Thãgba na kɔɔ cʋʋ kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩdaa dɩɩ do də̃bəələə?
46001021	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ Thãgbaa kpɛsɛ hanɩ, tibil na kɔɔ puno na ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ kpɛsɛ a jɩ Thãgba ga, mɛ̃ gɩ kɔɔ da Thãgba haar dɩ gba Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ də̃bəəlela a taana wɩrɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar;
46001022	Juifisɔ jɩɩn wɩ-n ƴaal, dɩ Gɩrɛkɩsɔ na-n yɩrna kpɛsɛ ƴaalɛ,
46001023	sɩ se wer, Kirisitiikɛ wɩ kɔɔ kpanɩ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra, ɔɔda sɩ-n mɩɩ, dɩ nɛ baradaa gɩ do Juifisɔra, a dona də̃bəəle wιrɛraakɛ na dɔnι Juifisɔa';
46001024	dι Kirisitira dɔ Thãgbaa fãga, na Thãgbaa kpɛsɛ, wιrɛraakɛ Thãgba wenι, ado Juifisɔ wɛ, ado Juifisɔ wa'.
46001025	Gιdonι gιrɛ hɔnι Thãgbaa də̃bəəl tibil yinəna, gι hananɛ kpɛsɛrɛ a jɔ tibilida, dι gιrɛ hɔnι Thãgbaa yɔɔ hana fãga a jɔ tibili fãga.
46001026	Nι hιnɛ omιna, mɔ̃kɛ werιkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ we nιnι hanι: Anι thɩ̃thιιn, wιrɛɛkɛ dɔnι tιι kpɛsɛsɔ tibil yinənaakɛ wa kpɛra', dι wιrɛ dɔnι fãgadara wa kpɛra', dι wιrɛ dɔnι dakha nũfe wa kpɛra';
46001027	sι Thãgba phiire gιrɛ tibil n wenι də̃bəəle ga-n pɛ kpɛsɛdarara yicuru. Thãgba phιire gɩrɛ tibil na-n thernana', ga-n pɛ fãgadarara yicuru;
46001028	Thãgba phiire gɩrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ irə', na gɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ-n beesini, kɛ na dɔnɩ thɩ̃a', gɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ gɩ debi gɩ do mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ,
46001029	dɩ mɛ̃ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na puno na məbi Thãgbaa ƴɛra ga.
46001030	Dɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛra dɔ nɔɔ dɩ nɩ ha gɩrɛ Jeju Kirisitira, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ Thãgba cʋʋnɩ dɩ do sar kpɛsɛrɛ, na fɩl sarʋ, na kpɩɩ leere, na birsere;
46001031	dɩ mɛ̃ gɩ ha mɔna gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ n məbəni, a na-n məbi gɩrɛraakɛ Kɔ̃tɩn cʋʋnɩ.”
46002001	Mɛrɛ dakha omɩna, ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ pɔnɩ anɩ pa, ga do thɩmɩɩ cʋno agɩbo kpɛsɛ kʋkʋʋ mɩ pɔna, a mɩɩna nɩ Thãgbaa sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩa';
46002002	gɩdonɩ ma kɔɔ ƴaal ɩ̃ jɛ thɩ̃ kpɩɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, saagado Jeju Kirisiti gι, kɛra wι kɔɔ kpanι thιrʋra gaaga.
46002003	Mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛrakɛ kɔɔ hanι anι pa, sʋmʋmʋ̃ mι kɔɔ ha, na maar na jẽu.
46002004	Dι ɩ̃ thιmιι na ɩ̃ Thãgba thιmιι mιι, ga kɔɔ do kpɛsɛ thιmιaakɛ dɔnι ha fidaa ga, sι thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛɛkɛ thɛnι Thu Phuu fãgara gι kɔɔ do,
46002005	dι mɛ̃ ga do tibil kpɛsɛrɛra anι ha pɛ dɛ̃a', sι Thãgbaa fãgara ga dɛ̃ɛ.
46002006	Sιrakɛ sι-n mιιrɛ kpɛsɛrɛ wιrɛraakɛ leanι gbιlgbιlgbιlι thɩ̃thιιn, sι ga do nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ kpɛsɛ ga, dι nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔkɛ na bũburonenii kpɛsɛ gι woa'.
46002007	Sι Thãgbaa kpɛsɛ sι-n mιι, kɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ gbul a dona thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ keranι, kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ maanι pɛrɛ sι aa kɔɔ ti yιɛr pa' aa, sι bulo kha na ɔɔ i dʋbι.
46002008	Dι kpɛsɛrɛ gιιkɛ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ na jιna', gιdonι adora wι kɔɔ jι gɛr, wa kɔɔ kpa Kɔ̃tιnɩkɛ hɩnanɩ i dʋbɩrɛ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra ga;
46002009	sɩ gɩ har mɔna gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ yire na kɔɔ yɩna', kɛ nũu na kɔɔ nɩɛna', dɩ ga kɔɔ jaa tibillə dɩ kpɩɛrna ga, gɛr Thãgba gbɛbɩ thɩɩn wɩrɛraakɛ n naanɛɛnɩ.”
46002010	Sɩ sɛr Thãgba kɔɔ gba ɔɔ Thu a nɩnana, gɩdonɩ Thu Phuu n 'lor thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ jɩ tue, narakɛ Thãgbaa thɩ̃ɩkɛ huloneni.
46002011	Gɩdonɩ, tibil ʋmɔ̃ na punone na jɩ tibildaa, saagado ntɛɛ thuukɛ hanɩ ɔɔ bɩnɔ ga? Mɛna gɩ, tibil na puno na jɩ Thãgbaada, saagado Thãgbaa Thu gaaga.
46002012	Sɩ se wer, gɩrɛ sɩ 'lɛnɩ ga do thɩdaa ga, sɩ Thueekɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara sɩ 'lɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ sa jɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ bɔ jɩɩrra.
46002013	Dɩ gɛrra sɩ-n mɩɩ dakha, sɩ ga do na thɩmɩɩ ca ƴɩrɛ kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩdaa n gbanɩ da-n dɩɩrna ga, sɩ mɔ̃kɛ thɩmɩɩ ca ƴɩrɛ Thu Phuu n dɩɩrnanɩ hanɩ, dɩ sɩ gbana dɩɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thudaa dɩ sa-n mɩɛ Thu Phuudara.
46002014	Sɩ tibilikɛ na hananɩ Thãgbaa Thuə', aa-n tu Thãgbaa Thu thã', gɩdonɩ də̃bəəle gɩ-n dʋʋraa, dɩ a na puno na jɩ ga, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa Thu n mɩɛnɛ gele.
46002015	Sɩ tibilikɛ hananɩ Thu Phuu, a-n jʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ jɩ gɩ, sɩ ɔr thɛthɛ tibil na jʋʋrʋʋ na jɩa';
46002016	dɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Amɛ kɔɔ jɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ kpɩɛr a punoo a dɩɩr thɩ̃ɛ?” Sɩ se wer sɩ hananɛ Kirisitii kpɩɛr.
46003001	Ado mɛr gɩ omɩna, ma kɔɔ puno a mɩɩna nɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n mɩɩnanɩ Thu Phuudara ga, sɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ donɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ hananɩ tibil kpɩɛrɛ dɩbara dɔrɔɔm, na mɔ̃kɛ nɩ donɩ bibɔrɔsɔ Kirisitira.
46003002	Ɩlɛ̃ mɩ kɔɔ ha nɩ ga do dɩko khena ga, gɩdonɩ na-n kɔɔ puno na mar pa', na nɛnɛ̃kɛrakɛ, sɩ na-n mar pa',
46003003	gɩdonɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ hananɩ tibil kpɩɛrɛ dɩbara dɔrɔɔm nɩ do 'lo. Gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ gbugi na kɩla n bonɩ dɩ ga-n ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, ga do tɩbɩlaakɛ hananɩ tibil kpɩɛrɛ dɩbara dɔrɔɔm nɩ do dɩ na-n ɩɩr a ho tɩɩ ba gaa?
46003004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ ʋ n sonɩ dɩ yɩ, ine wer Polɩda ɩnɩ do; ʋ n yɩ, ine wer Apolɔsɩɩda ɩnɩ do, na thʋ̃ do tɩbɩlaakɛ hananɩ tibil kpɩɛrɛ dɩbara dɔrɔɔm mãa?
46003005	Anye Apolɔsɩ do? Dɩ anye Pol do? Thɔ̃dara wɩ do, kɛ dɔnɩ nɔɔ dɩ nɩ pɛr haar, mɔ̃kɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ha wɩnɩ bɩɛlbɩɛl thɔma.
46003006	Mɛr kɔɔ dire, dɩ Apolɔsɩ sɛ, sɩ Thãgba n cʋɛ dɩ ga-n khɔ̃;
46003007	mɛ̃ gɩɩ, ga do ʋrɛ n direni dʋɔn thɩ̃ɛ dɩ ʋrɛ n sɛnɩ ga, sɩ Thãgbaakɛ n cʋɛnɩ dɩ ga-n khɔ̃ gɩ.
46003008	Ʋrɛ n direni, na ʋrɛ n sɛnɩ, bɛla wɩ do, dɩ wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl na 'lɛr awɩ thɛthɛɛ lɩmɩ mɔ̃ awɩ thɛthɛɛ thɔ̃ hanɩ.
46003009	Gɩdonɩ thɔ̃ dona sɩ do nakha Thãgba, dɩ nɩ dor Thãgbaa lɛ, a dona Thãgbaa cɔ.
46003010	Mɔ̃kɛ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ mɩnɩ hanɩ, mɩ kɔɔ kpɛɛ gʋʋ mɔ̃kɛ go mɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ kpɛsɛɛ n kpɛɛnɩ gʋʋ, dɩ tibil kpɩɩ n dɛbɩ. Sɩ dɔ tɩbɩla bɩɛlbɩɛl n jɩɩ hɩɩn mɔ̃ wɩ-n dɛbɩnɩ;
46003011	gɩdonɩ tibil na bir na kpɛɛ go kpɩɩ, saagado gɩrɛ kɔɔ 'lenɩ kpɛɛrɛ gaaga, gɛr dʋɔn Jeju Kirisiti.
46003012	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ado tibil na dɛbɩ go kpɛɛrɛɛkɛ na dɛ, na dɛ bulo, na boka ɓɔnaakɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ, na dɛɛ, na hʋɔn, na thagbola,
46003013	ga yɩrrɛ dɩ wa jɩ mɔ̃ tɩbɩla bɩɛlbɩɛlɩ thɔ̃ hanɩ. Gɩdonɩ Wireele na nɛrɔ, gɩdonɩ dɔɔ na nɛrɔ, dɩ dɔɔlera na mɩɛnɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛlɩ thɔ̃ na hɩɩn.
46003014	Ado ntɛɛ thɔ̃ɔkɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ a dɛbɩnɩ go kpɛɛrɛraale bo sɩ, ga dor a na 'lɛr lɩmιnɛ;
46003015	sι ado dɔɔ hɩ̃ ntɛɛ thɔ̃, ga dor a 'leere, sι ɔɔ thɛthɛ wer na 'lɛr taarɛ, sι ga hor dɔɔra a ca the.
46003016	Na jι dιι do nɛr dɔ cʋɔr Thãgbara, dι Thãgbaa Thu na-n cɔ anι bιnɔaa?
46003017	Ado tibil wɩɛl Thãgbaa cɔ, Thãgba na wɩɛlʋʋlɛ; gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa cɔ n phure, dɩ nɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa cɔra.
46003018	Tibil na-n fɩɩl dɩbara ga. Ado tibil anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn na kpɩɛr ɩnɛr dʋɔn tɩɩ kpɛsɛ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛ, a ka deba dɔ də̃bəəlu dɩ mɛ̃ a na do tɩɩ kpɛsɛ.
46003019	Gɩdonɩ kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩdaa də̃bəəle gɩ do Thãgbara, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “A fʋrɛ tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔra awɩ fɩɩlla”;
46003020	wo: “Kɔ̃tɩn jɩrɛ tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔɔ kpɩɛr, a jɩ gɛr dɩɩ do mɔlɔdaa gɩ do.”
46003021	Gɛr gɩ tibil na-n gba tibil a do ɔɔ mə̃bida ga, gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ nɛr hɩna,
46003022	ado Pol gɩ, ado Apolɔsɩ gɩ, ado Sefasɩ gɩ, ado thιɩkɛɛda gɩ, ado yire gɩ, ado khir gɩ, ado nɛnɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ gɩ, ado thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na ɩnanι gι, thɩ̃ɛ ɓibi nɛr hιna.
46003023	Sι nɛrɛ Kirisiti hιna nι, sι Kirisiti Thãgba hιnaa.
46004001	Dɔ wa-n hιιn sι mɔ̃kɛ sι donι Kirisitii thɔ̃dara, na wιrɛ Thãgba pɛrnι wa-n dɔna ɔɔ thɩ̃ gbul thɔma;
46004002	sι a thιɛna gaa mɔ̃ wι-n ƴaalnιnakɛ thɔ̃ donaale n hana dʋɔn, dɔ wι do sobɔ cʋʋdara.
46004003	Sι ado mɛrra gι, dι na hιιn mι jʋjʋʋr hιιnʋʋ yo, dι agιbo tibil n kιlɛna mι kιιl paar yo, ga ba mι fιιʋraka', dι mɛrɛrakɛ ma laar nayι ɩ̃ yɛ dιι dιbara ga,
46004004	gιdonι ma jιna mι hananɛ bara paar dιkhara fιιʋraka'; sι ga nιna dι mι 'leere dι paar phuphulə', ʋrɛ na kιlɛna mιnι Kɔ̃tιn gι.
46004005	Gɛr gι bɔɔ na danι pa', na-n 'laa na yι dιa', na-n pιɛrɛ Kɔ̃tιn a ɩ̃, ʋrɛɛkɛ na cʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ keranɩ dɩ a the dahɩrɛra, kɛ na nɛrɔnɩ dakha gɩrɛ haar n kpɩɛrnanɩ, liir tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl na 'lɛ Thãgbara khɩɩrɛɛkɛ teana wɩnɩ.
46004006	Omɩna, nɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ gba ɩ̃ thɛthɛ na Apolɔsιιda a mιιna nι thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ, dι mɛ̃ asιdaakɛ na dιιrnι, dι na kpãsɛ gιrɛraakɛ kherenena', gι ho tibil bιɛl na hananɛ ʋ saa bo ʋa'.
46004007	Gιdonι amɛ cʋɛ fι dι fι ha kpιι? Anye fι hana, sι ga do wι kɔɔ ha fɛra? Dι ado wι kɔɔ ha fɛr, mɔ̃gιdo dr fa-n məbi ga-n ho wι kɔɔ ha fɛra?
46004008	Nι 'lire hiir waa phi; nι 'lire dʋʋr lɛ̃lɛ; jaa fãgadara nɩ do gɩrɛ, sɩ ser na halaa koe. Ɩ̃ ƴaal werrakɛ dʋɔn nɩ dɔ fãgadara, dɩ mɛ̃ sa bul kha na nɛrɛ fãgadaar dʋʋrra.
46004009	Mee gɩ hʋrɛ Thãgba ka thɩɩnɛ sɛr thɔ̃thɔna, dɩ sɩ do pɩpɩra, dɩ sa-n hona wɩrɛ teananɩ kʋʋrɛ, gɩdonɩ sɩ kɔɔ debire a do fɛʋra yi ga thɩ̃ɛ, Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔra na tɩbɩlala.
46004010	Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sɩ do də̃bələ, sɩ ne wer ka do tɩɩ kpɛsɛsɔ Kirisitira; sɛr yɔɔ, sɩ ner ka do dakhena; wɩ-n cʋrɛ ne wer, sɩ se wer wɩ-n beesi ser.
46004011	A dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ, sɩ-n gaarɛ kɔmɛrra, na yɔlkhaara, sɩ ha kẽkẽ bʋɔ, bɩɩr haar wɩ-n bɩɩr sɩ, sa hana cɔ gʋa';
46004012	sa-n vɔɔ asɩ nyɛ̃ thɔna kpãkpalã woa'; wɩ-n nɩɩr sɛr sɩ sa-n bɔna wɩ; wɩ-n kpoo sarɛ sɩ sa-n fʋ haar;
46004013	wɩ-n kʋɛ sɛr ire sɩ ser n mɩɩna wɛr na hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ; sɩ kɔɔ debire a ho tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩraa sɔ̃sʋɔn, a hona tɩbɩla fɛʋra puuyʋʋ a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ.
46004014	Ga do mɩ khere narɛ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ gɩ cʋɛ yicuru gɩ fʋ na', sι fιlɛ mι-n dιιr nι, mɔ̃kɛ nι donι ɩ̃ bιsãsɔɔkɛ mι-n nanι.
46004015	Gιdonι adorakɛ nɩ hananɛ dɩɩrdara gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr Kirisitiidara, sɩ na hana thɛ wer jɔa', gɩdonɩ mɛr gɩɩkɛ kɔna nɩnɩ Jeju Kirisitira, dɩɩ the tutugo bʋɔra.
46004016	Gɛr gɩ mɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr nɩ dɔ ɩ̃ phɛldara.
46004017	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ thɔ̃ nar Timothe ɩ̃ bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ sobɔ tibil Kɔ̃tɩnna, ɔr na cʋɛ nɩ dɩ na jɩ mɔ̃ ɩ̃ ɩɩr pa hanɩ na Kirisiti, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ we gbɛbɩdara fɛʋ paar fɛʋ.
46004018	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ nɛrɛra n kar ire dɩɩ ho ma pɔ la'.
46004019	Sɩ ado Kɔ̃tɩn tu, kɩɛr na gbe ma pɔr, sɩ ga do i kadaraa nɔfa thɩmɩɩ mɩ-n ƴaal ɩ̃ ja', sɩ awɩ fãga.
46004020	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa fãgadaar do, ga do nɔfaarra gɩ ha ga, sɩ fãga wɩ-n yɩ.
46004021	Anye nɩ-n ƴaal? Ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa na ciləmũu yaa, agɩbo ɩ̃ pɔ na naʋ na hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ?
46005001	Wɩ-n mɩɩrɛ paar fɛʋ ayɩ, bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ n har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ bɔdɛl cʋʋ caakɛ na-n hanɩnakɛ thɩldaraa pa gaa gɩ, dɩ tibil bɩɛl ba gbananakɛ ɔɔ thɩɩ khɛr.
46005002	Sɩ dɩ nɩ borakɛ sɩ na ka iree. Mee bʋɔ ka teena gɩ fɔ nɩ, wɩ ti tibil ca ole cʋɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ thale a hɛllɔ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
46005003	Sɩ ado me wer ma hanɩ kha na nɛrɛ tomɩrra gbelẽ gbelã', sɩɩ do thue haan kha na nɛrɛ, mɩ 'lire kɩɩlna tibilile cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃ caale pɩ, dɩɩ ho mɩ kɔɔ hale.
46005004	Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ iikɛ sɩ-n gbɛbɩrɔnɩ kha, dɩ ɩ̃ thu n hale, dɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ fãga n ha kha na sɛrɛ,
46005005	nɩ dɔ tibil ca ole n do ʋrɛ wɩ-n faanɩ ha Satã, a kʋɛsʋʋ tomɩr, dɩ mɛ̃ ɔɔ thu na 'lɛ taarɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wirə.
46005006	Khaar nɩ-n məbi mɔlɔ; na jɩ dɩɩ do tabɩɩr fɩɩʋ n cʋʋrɛ buru mɩ̃ boloo fɛʋ dɩɩ bʋ̃aa?
46005007	Nɩ cʋɛ tabɩ tɩ̃ɩ gɩ buur, dɩ mɛ̃ na do buru mɩ̃ bolo phaa, gɩ the gɩrɛraakɛ na hananɩ tabɩɩra'; gɩdonɩ wɩ jinəne Kirisiti asɩ Pakɩ bana bi bonɩɛ.
46005008	Gɛr gɩ sa-n cʋɛ fɛtɩɩle ga-n do na tabɩ tɩ̃a', na tabɩɩrɩkɛ hananɩ puu cʋʋrɛ dɩ kpallɛ ga, sɩ gɩ dɔ buruukɛ tabɩɩr na harna', gɛr dʋɔn phur nakha sobɔr.
46005009	Mɩ kɔɔ kherere ɩ̃ sɛbɛra a ha nɩ ayɩ: Na-n bɔ kha na bɔdɛl cʋʋdara ga.
46005010	Sɩ ga do waa bɔdɛl cʋʋdaraakɛ hanɩ thɩɩraakɛ ba, na ha pɩɛrdara, na tɩɩ tagɩrɩdara, na thɩldara mɩ soa', gɩdonɩ ado thale gɩ, ga dor gɩ teenanɛ nɩ thɩɩr thɩɩraakɛ.
46005011	Sɩ gɩrɛ mɩ khere narnɩ gɩrɛ dʋɔn wɔɔ: Na-n bɔ kha na tibilikɛ yɛnɩ omine ha nɩ, sa do bɔdɛl cʋʋdaar, agɩbo ha pɩɛrdaara', dɩ agɩbo thɩl a hana, dɩ agɩbo tɩɩ nɩɩrdaar ga, agɩbo ta laardaar gɩ, na tɩɩ tagɩrɩdaara'; na-n kho kha dɩkorrakɛ na tibil ca ola'.
46005012	Gɩdonɩ anye mɩ ha kha na tɩɩ khɩna a na kɩɩlna wɩ? Ga do wɩrɛ nɩ donanɩ kha pa bɩɛldara na kɩɩlna gaa?
46005013	Mee gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Nɩ te tɩɩ puu anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a faa.” Ado wɩrɛ dɔnɩ tɩɩ khɩna wɛ, Thãgba na kɩlɛna wɩ.
46006001	Ado ʋ̃ tibil anɩ ha hananɛ sor na ʋ, a na 'lar na wɩɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgba na hɛllɔnɩ soraa pa wɩ kɩlɛnaa ya, ga do tɩɩ phuusɔɔ pa ga gʋʋraa?
46006002	Na jɩ dɩɩ do tɩɩ phuusɔ na kɩlɛna thɩ̃ tinənəə? Dɩ ado nɛr na kɩlɛna thɩ̃ tinəne, na thʋ̃ na mar na kɩɩl kɩɩl yɩra gaa?
46006003	Na jɩ dɩɩ do sɛr na kɩlɛna thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔaa? Dɩ a thale gɩ, sa teena sɩ kɩɩl nɛnɛ̃ yireekɛɛ kɩɩlaa?
46006004	Sɩ a nɩ hana kha sor nɛnɛ̃ yireekɛɛ thɩmɩɩra, dɩɩ do tɩbɩlaakɛ we gbɛbɩdara na-n thernana' nɩ-n ƴaal wɩ gʋrɛ gɩ.
46006005	Mɩ mɩɩrɛ gɩrɛ yicuru n fɔ nɩ, dɩ ger ha mɛnakɛ, tɩɩ bɩɛl na ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a hana kpɛsɛrɛ, a gʋʋr ɔɔ omisɔɔ soaa?
46006006	Sɩ dɩ ʋ̃ omi n hana ʋ̃ omi sor, dɩɩ ba jal na jɩɩl ha pɛ 'leedaraa ƴɛra?
46006007	Sobɔr gɩ, sopugo 'lire ka nar mɔ̃kɛ nɩ-n kɩɩlnɩ khasɔ. Mɔ̃gɩdo a ga ha otə' dɩ na-n tu la? Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ na-n tu anɩda n jala ga?
46006008	Sɩɩ do nɛr n ka na-n cʋʋ gιrɛ na-n hanι otə', dι nι yι tιbιlaada n ka na jala, dι omιnana nι-n cʋʋrakɛ gelela wo.
46006009	Na jι dιι do wιrɛ na sarana na lõ Thãgba fãgadaarι dʋɔaa gaa? Na-n fιιl dιbara ga: Bɔdɛl cʋʋdara, na thιldara, na khɛ kpιι ƴaaldara na kũu kpιι ƴaaldara, na wιrɛ n cʋɛnι khɛr khaa, na konaakɛ n ƴaalɛnι kuun khɛr khaa, na khɛraakɛ n ƴaalɛnι khɛr kuun kha,
46006010	na yudara, na ha pιɛrdara, na ta laardara, na tιι nιιrdara, na tιι tagιrιdara, wa lõ Thãgba fãgadaarι dʋɔa'.
46006011	Dι thalera ιkhaa tibilsɔ nɛrɛra kɔɔ ha, sι Thãgba kɔɔ cɔcɔɔ nɛr, a kɔɔ lee ner kpιι, a kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ sor dιι hɛl nar dιι do Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιnι i na asι Thãgbaa Thu dɔ nɔɔ.
46006012	Nι yι, hʋɛ hale thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ cʋʋra, sobɔr gɩ wer, sɩ ga do thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na dɔ nar thɩ̃ bʋɔa'. Mɩ hananɛ hʋɛ wer a na cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, sι ma tu kpιιrakɛ a na do thɩ̃ bιɛlι dea'.
46006013	Dιkor dʋɔn bιnɛɛda, dι dakha bιnɛ do dιkorιda; sι Thãgba na kperẽ ger fɛʋ a na kʋɛ. Sι Thãgba na kɔɔ cʋʋ tomɩr bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra ga, sɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda tomɩr do, dɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ tomɩrɩda gɩ bar Kɔ̃tɩn.
46006014	Dɩ Thãgbaakɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn khirera, na ɩɩr sɛr dakha na ɔɔ fãga.
46006015	Na jɩ dɩɩ do anɩ tomɩ dʋɔn Kirisitii tomɩ ɓã gaa? Dɩ ma gbaar Kirisitii tomɩ ɓã wo ɩ̃ cʋʋ gɩ do khɛ bɔdɛlɩ tomɩ ɓã ya? Kpei, ga-n ha thalaa koe.
46006016	Na jɩ dɩɩ do ʋrɛɛkɛ lenɩ kha na khɛ bɔdɛl, tomɩ bɩɛl wɩ gbɛbɩ do kha gaa? Gɩdonɩ gɩ sor Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Wɛr yenyɔ na debire na do tibil bɩɛl.”
46006017	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ lenɩ kha na Kɔ̃tɩn wɩ gbɛbɩrɛ do kha thu bɩɛl.
46006018	Nɩ fe khiru pɛ bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra. Sopugo wo sopugookɛ tibil n cʋʋnɩ, ga-n lʋ̃ʋ tomɩrra ga, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ faanɩ dɩbara bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra, ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ tomɩra a-n cʋʋ sopugo da-n pɛ.
46006019	Na jɩ dɩɩ do anɩ tomɩ dʋɔn cʋɔr Thu Phuurəəkɛ hanɩ anɩ bɩnɔ, kɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ Thãgbara gaa? Na hɩ̃ anɩbara ga.
46006020	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba kɔɔ the ner the nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka, gɛr gɩ anɩ tomɩra na anɩ thurə nɩ cʋɛ Thãgbaa i ga-n dʋbɩrɔ.
46007001	Ado gɩrɛraakɛ nɩ kɔɔ khere marnɩ gɩ, gɩ bɔrɛ tibillə dɩ a na-n tha khɛrra ga.
46007002	Sɩ mɔ̃ ga fʋnɩ sɩ bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ na-n hala', dɔ kuun n hana ɔɔ khɛr ker, khɛr n hana ɔɔ ko ker.
46007003	Dɔ kuun na-n ha ɔɔ khɛr gɩrɛɛkɛ teanaanɩ, khɛr na-n cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃ dakha ɔɔ kora.
46007004	Khɛr na hɩ̃ ɔɔ tomɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ kuun hɩna; mɛna gɩ, kuun na hɩ̃ ɔɔ tomɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ khɛr hɩna.
46007005	Na-n bo kha phɩɩn, saagado nɔ bɩɛl nɩ gʋʋr kha sa lee kha gbe, nɩ yɩ ƴιɛ Thãgba bɩɛlɛla gaaga; sɩ agɩpɩ nɩ bir nɩ gbɛbɩ, a mɛ̃ gaa Satã na yɩrɛ hʋɛ na fifilə ni, gɩrɛraakɛ na marnɩ na fʋ dɩbara ga.
46007006	Mɔ̃ mɩ yɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ ha thakɛ gɛrra mɩ so, sɩ ga do jɔfʋ gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ pɛra',
46007007	sɩ ga da marɛ ado tɩbɩla fɛʋ na har mɔ̃kɛ mɩ hanɩ; sɩ tɩbɩla bɩɛlbɩɛl hananɛ khaardaa dɩɩdɩɩkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa, ʋ n hana ɔɔda kpɩɩ, ʋ na ɔɔda kpɩɩ.
46007008	Sɩ ado wɩrɛɛkɛ na hɛnɩ pa', na khikhɛra, mer yɩ gɩ bɔrɛ wɩ tɔɔ mɔ̃kɛ mɩ hanɩ.
46007009	Sɩ ado wa mar na fʋ dɩbara ga, dɔ wɩ he, gɩdonɩ her baar thueekɛ na fɔ wɩnɩ ga-n hərə wi.
46007010	Sɩ ado wɩrɛ hɛnɩ pɩ gɩ, jɔfʋ gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ pɛr, sɩ ga do mɛr jɛ gɩ pɛra', Kɔ̃tɩn sɔ, dɩ khɛr na-n bo ɔɔ koa'.
46007011	Sι ado a 'lire bor, a tɔɔ a na-n he tιι kpιι bã, agιbo wι gʋrɛ kha sa a bir a gba ɔɔ ko; sι kuun na-n faa ɔɔ khɛra'.
46007012	Sι mι sor wɩ̃ tibilsɔra ga do Kɔ̃tιn ga, sι ɩ̃ pa gι the: Ado õkuun hananɛ khɛrιkɛ na pιɛrnι haara', sι khɛr dɔɔ tu ιna toore na ιnι ko, kuun na-n fagʋa'.
46007013	Sι a khɛr hana kuun daa pɛr haara', sa tu a toona khɛr dɔɔ, khɛrɩle na-n faa ɔɔ kora ga.
46007014	Gɩdonɩ kuunikɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haara', khɛr n dor nɔɔ dɩ tiro dɩ ha kpɩɩ; dɩ khɛrɩkɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haara', õkuun n dor nɔɔ dɩ tiro dɩ ha kpɩɩ; a ga ha thala', ga dor anɩ bɩsãsɔ na hor thɩldaar bɩsana, sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ wɩ tirore ha kpɩɩ.
