46007015	Sɩ ado ʋrɛɛkɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haara' ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n bo a punone bo; a õkuun gɩ, a õkhɩɛn gɩ, liir dɩphã li paar na hala', gɩdonɩ ha ie toorera Thãgba we sɩ.
46007016	Gɩdonɩ khɛr, mɔ̃ fɩ jɩ dɩ fɛr na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ afɩ ko na 'lɛrɔ taarɛ? Dɩ agɩbo kuun, mɔ̃ fɩ jɩ dɩ fɛr na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ afɩ khɛr na 'lɛrɔ taarɛ?
46007017	Gele hale gbobi, sɩ tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩɩ na-n jala mɔna Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ yɩnɩ gɩ hana, gɩ mɩɛna mɔ̃ Thãgba wenɩ ntɛ; thakɛ mɩ pɛr gɩ hana we gbɛbɩdarara paar fɛʋ.
46007018	Tibil hale dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ wɩɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a donɩ khʋ̃ kurdaar ya? A na-n kerroa'. Tibil hale dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ wɩɩ sɩ aa 'lɛ kur khʋ̃a ya? Ntɛ na-n kur khʋ̃ʋ bã.
46007019	Khʋ̃ kurre na do thɩ̃a', a fa kur khʋ̃a', ga do thɩ̃ɛ dakha ga, sɩ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛ gɛr dɔ thɩ̃ɛ.
46007020	Tibil n tɔɔ mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ hanɩ sɩ dɩ Thãgba wɩɩ.
46007021	Dee fɩ kɔɔ do sɩ dɩ Thãgba we fɩ ya? Fa-n dɛna ga; sɩ ado fɩ yɩ hʋɛ wer a na do waʋ, ka gba hʋ dɔɔle.
46007022	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ dee, sɩ dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn wɩɩ, Kɔ̃tɩnɩ waʋ a do; dɩ mɛ̃ ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ waʋ, sɩ dɩ Thãgba wɩɩ, Kirisitii dee a do.
46007023	Thãgba kɔɔ the ner the nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka, na-n debi do tɩbɩlaa dea'.
46007024	Omɩna, mɔ̃kɛ nɩ kɔɔ hanɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ we nɩnɩ dɩɩdɩɩ, mɛ̃ na too kha na Thãgba.
46007025	Sɩ ado wɩrɛ dɔnɩ khɛ biirəəkɛ na jɛnɩ kuunaa gɩ, ma hana jɔfʋʋkɛ thɛnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ pa ga, sɩ ɩ̃ kpɩɛrnɔ mɩ-n ha nɩ, mɔ̃kɛ mɩ donɩ tibilikɛ Kɔ̃tɩn donanɩ bʋɔ dɩ ɩ̃ do sobɔ tibil.
46007026	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n kpɩɛrnɩ gɛr bʋɔnɔ, gɩdonɩ bɔɔkɛra n ɩnanɩ khɩɩrɛ: Gɩ bɔrɛ dɩ tibil na too mɔ̃kɛ a hanɩ.
46007027	Fɩ lire kha na khɛr ya? Fa-n ƴaal fɩ kuure lidaala'; a fa hana khɛra', fa-n yɩ fɩ hɛ khɛra'.
46007028	Sɩ ado fɩ her, ga do sopugo fɩ cʋa'; sɩ ado khɛ biireekɛ na jɛnɩ kuuna' he kuun, ga do sopugo a cʋa'. Sɩ wɩrɛ hɛnɩ, wa yɩrɛ nɩwɛ awɩ yi hanana, dɩ ma-n na nɩ yɛ ga nɩɩlera ga.
46007029	Sɩ mɩ yɩ wɔɔ omɩnaa: Bɔɔra 'lire paalɛ, dɔ dɩphã wɩrɛ hananɩ khɛr n ho wɩrɛ na hananɩ khɛra ga;
46007030	dɩ wɩrɛ n bɛnɩ n ho wɩrɛ na-n bɛna'; dɔ wɩrɛ n kãkanɛnɩ n ho wɩrɛ na-n kãkanɛna', dɩ wɩrɛ n thɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ n ho wɩrɛ na hananɩ thɩ̃a';
46007031	dɔ wɩrɛ n 'lɛnɩ awɩda thɩɩraakɛ n ho wɩrɛ na-n 'lɛnɩ thɩ̃a'; gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ thɩɩra hanɩ gɩrɛ, a-n phor.
46007032	Sɩ mɩ nar na-n dɛ fɩɩʋraka'. Ʋrɛɛkɛ na hɛnɩ khɛra', Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩ̃ a-n dɛna, mɔ̃ a na fʋnɩ sɩ na da Kɔ̃tɩn haar.
46007033	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ hɛnɩ khɛr, thɩɩkɛɛda a-n dɛna, mɔ̃ a na fʋnɩ sɩ na da ɔɔ khɛr haar,
46007034	dɩ ƴɩɛ yenyɔ a-n jɛ. Khɛrɩkɛ na hananɩ kuuna' na khɛ biireekɛ na jɛnɩ kuuna', Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩ̃ wɩ-n dɛna ɩnɩ-n pho tomɩrra na thuerə. Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ hɛnɩ kuun, thɩɩkɛɛda a-n dɛna, mɔ̃ a na fʋnɩ sɩ na da ɔɔ ko haar.
46007035	Mɔ̃ mɩ-n mɩɩnɩ thakɛ, anɩda bɔ mɩ-n ƴaal, ga do pheru mɩ-n pɛ nara', sɩ fɩl bʋɔ mɩ-n nɩ nar, dɩ na jɩɩ hɩɩn nɩ faa dɩbara Kɔ̃tɩnna, dɩ dɩkha na hale na dĩdiə na'.
46007036	Sɩ ado tibil yɩɛ dɩɩ do ga dor i kʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ ɔɔ khɛ biirrəəkɛ na jɛnɩ kuuna', ado ɔɔ he bɔ na ka, dɩ kpɩɛr a yɩɛ dɩɩ bɔr herra, a cʋɛ gɩrɛ a yɩnɩ dɩɩ bɔr, ga do sopugo a cʋa'; dɔ her n cʋʋ.
46007037	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kpɩɛrɛnɩ hi ɔɔ bɩnɔ dɩ ga do fɛrɛrɛ ga, sɩɩ do dɩbara a fʋ ayɩ, ɩna mar ɩnɩ khɛ biirrəəkɛ na jɛnɩ kuuna' da too, ntɛɛle cʋʋrɛ bɔɔ.
46007038	Mɛ̃ gι, ʋrɛɛkɛ faanι ɔɔ khɛ biirikɛ na jɛnι kuuna' dι he kuun, a cʋʋrɛ bɔɔ, sι ʋrɛɛkɛ na tuonni ιnι khɛ biir n hɛ kuuna', a cʋʋrɛ bɔɔ a jɔ.
46007039	Khɛr n lire kha na ɔɔ ko bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ ɔɔ ko hananι yire; sι a ɔɔ ko khi, a hananɛ hʋɛ na he ʋrɛɛkɛ a-n ƴaalnι, sι dɔ gι do mɔ̃ Kɔ̃tιn tuni.
46007040	Sι ado mɔ̃ ɩ̃ kpιɛrnɔ hanι gι, ado a too mɔ̃kɛ a hanι ga daaraarɛ na jɔ, dι mι pɛrɛ haar Thãgbaa Thu wer mι hanaanɛ.
46008001	Sι ado bonι ji nʋ̃daara gι, sι jιrɛ wer sɛrɛ fɛʋ hananɛ jιιr, sι jιιr n 'laarɛ i kaar, sι naʋ n cʋɛ dι tibil n khɔ̃ da-n pɛr.
46008002	Ado tibil pɛr haar ιnι jιrɛ thɩ̃ɛ, aa jι gι mɔ̃ gι teenanι a jɛ ga.
46008003	Sι ado tibil na Thãgba, tibil ole Thãgba jιιrɛ dakha.
46008004	Sι ado bonι ji nʋ̃ khodaara gι, sι jιrɛ dι thιl na do thɩ̃ɛ thιιra ga, dι thãgba kpιι na hale saagado bιɛl gι dιbara gaaga.
46008005	Gιdonι adorakɛ gιrɛ wι-n wenι thãgbasɔ hale, a ƴũ gι a thιιra gι, gι hale wer a do thãgbasɔ jɔɔ na kɔ̃tιnasɔ jɔɔ.
46008006	Sι ado serra wer, Thãgba bιɛl dιbara haanle, a do Thιrɛɛkɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ theronι, ɔr te sι sι dɔ ɔɔda. Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιɛl dιbara haanle dakha, Jeju Kirisiti gι, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ harɔnι, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ sι doronι tibil.
46008007	Sι ga do tιbιla fɛʋ hana ga jιιla'; gιdonι ιkhasɔ kɔɔ mιlnanɛ thιla a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ, wι-n bor dι wa-n hιιnnakɛ nʋʋnιle wι-n khonι dɩɩ bo do bonɩ ji nʋʋnna 'lo, dɩɩ do mɛ̃ awɩ kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ na tɩɛnna' n cʋʋ wɩ dɩ wɩ ba pɛr haar nʋ̃ khorɩle pɛ narɛ dɩɩ.
46008008	Ga do dɩkor na cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sa 'li kha na Thãgba ga. A sa kho dɩkora', dɩkha na ɓɔr sa'; a sa kho, dɩkha na-n dɛbɩ sar woa'.
46008009	Sɩ na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn, dɩ anɩ hʋ hana na-n do nɛ baradaa wɩrɛraakɛ yɔɔna'.
46008010	Gɩdonɩ ado tibil yɩ fɩ, fɛrkɛ hananɩ jɩɩr, dɩ fɩ too bonɩ ji paar a na kho thɩ̃ɛ, tibilikɛ na tɩɛnnɩ ɔɔ kpɩɛrnɔra ga, ga do ga thɔgʋʋrɛ na pɛr da kho bonɩ ji nʋʋnna orraa?
46008011	Dɩ thale afɩ jɩra na cʋʋ ʋrɛ yɔɔnɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ omineekɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ khironi, da bu.
46008012	Dɩ a na cʋʋ sopugo thale omɩnana, a na cʋʋ awɩ kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ na tɩɛnna', dɩ a bũburõ, Kirisitira nɩ-n cʋʋ sopugo.
46008013	Dɩ gɛr gɩ, ado dɩkor na cʋɛ ɩ̃ omi da bara, ma kho nʋʋn kpɩɩrakɛ, gɩ ba cʋʋ ɩ̃ omi a bara ga.
46009001	Ma hana hʋɛ na cʋʋ mɔ̃ mι pɛrnι haaraa? Ga do thɔ̃thɔn ha maa? Ma kɔɔ yι Jeju asι Kɔ̃tãa? Ga do nɛr dɔ ɩ̃ nyɛ̃kιɛr thɔ̃ Kɔ̃tιnna gaa?
46009002	Ado ma do thɔ̃thɔn ιkhasɔra ga, sι ne wer mι thʋnɛ do nar thɔ̃thɔn, gιdonι nɛr dɔ jιιnιkɛ n nɛnanι dι thɔ̃thɔn ha mι, gιrɛraakɛ nι donι Kɔ̃tιnιda.
46009003	Gɛr dɔ ɩ̃ birseekɛ mι-n birseni wɛkɛ n pɛ marnι sor.
46009004	Sa hana hʋɛ sι kho sa-n yɔna gaa?
46009005	Sa hana hʋɛ na kpa ha pɛdaarιkɛ dɔnι asι khɛr sa-n kpaarna, mɔ̃kɛ wɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔna n cʋʋnɩ, na mɔ̃kɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ õkuunsɔ na Sefasι n cʋʋnaa?
46009006	Dɩ agɩbo mɛrra dɩbara na Barnabasɩ, ser na hana hʋɛ na ba faa asɩ nyɛ̃kɩɛr thɔ̃ dora gaa yaa?
46009007	Amɛ na gbaan ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ war a na-n lɩmɩ dɩbara sɩ a na-n cʋʋ sɔrasɩ? Amɛ na kʋlɛ lɩɛ sa a na kho ga thã? Amɛ na-n khɛ nʋma sɩ ga do nʋmaa ilẽ n haanɛa?
46009008	Gɩrɛ mɩ sonɩ, tibil kpɩɛrɛ gɩ dɩbara ya? Ga do thalera jɔfʋ soaa?
46009009	Mee gɩ kherere Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋra ayɩ: “Nakɩɩrɩkɛ na-n sanɩ jɔ, fa-n lii nʋɔa'.” Nakena Thãgba n kpɩɛrna dɩbara ya?
46009010	Agɩbo, ga do sɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩɩ mɩɩrɔ thalaa yaa? Ɔɔ, sɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩɩ kherero ayɩ: Ʋrɛɛkɛ n kʋlɛnɩ a teenanɛ a na-n kʋlɛ na nũ pɛrɛ, dɩ ʋrɛ na-n thɔnɩ jɔ, a na-n thɔ na nũ pɛrɛ mɔ̃ a na yɩrɔnɩ ɔɔda.
46009011	Ado sɩ kɔɔ diire anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thudaa, ga dor thɩ̃ kʋkʋʋ ado sa 'lɛ nar nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ thɩ̃sɔa bɛ?
46009012	Ado ʋkhasɔ hananɛ hʋɛ a na 'lɛ nar thɩ̃ɛ, ga do sɛr ka teena gaa? Sɩ sa kɔɔ cʋʋ mɔ̃kɛra sɩ hananɩ hʋɛa', sɩ sɩ-n fʋrɛ haar thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, dɩ mɛ̃ sa var Kirisitii tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ ga-n kpaaraa ga.
46009013	Na jɩ dɩɩ do wɩrɛɛkɛ n dɔnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ thɔma, thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n thɛnɩ Thãgba fʋɔr cʋɔrɔ wɩ-n khoaa? Na wɩrɛ n jenɩ bonɩɛ, bonɩ ji thɩɛna n haanɛ waa?
46009014	Dɩ mɛna Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ pɛr oti, dɩ wɩrɛ n mɩanɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, tutugo bʋɔ na-n haanɛ wɩ.
46009015	Sɩ mɛrɛ ma kɔɔ cʋʋrakɛ dɩɩ ho mɩ hananɛ ga hʋʋla'. Sɩ ma khere nar gɩrɛ nɩ cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃ mɛrɛra gaa koe, gɩdonɩ khir ka ba marɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ tibil na cʋʋnɩ dɩ a tɔ̃ mɩ ga məbiile.
46009016	Gɩdonɩ ado ma mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, ga do mar məbidaa ga; gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ gιιkɛ teananɩ ɩ̃ cʋɛ phubi, dɩ ga puu marɛ ado ma-n mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩa'.
46009017	Sɩ ado ɩ̃ ƴaalla gɩ the, ma 'lɛr lɩmɩnɛ; sɩ ado ga the ɩ̃ ƴaalla ga, thɔma gɩ a heen mι.
46009018	Dι anye dɔrakɛ ɩ̃ lιmɩ tɔr? Gɛr dɔ mɔ̃ mɩ-n mɩɩnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, ɩ̃ mɩa gɩ na 'laanɛ khaar, sι ma-n bo na kpãkpãa hʋ hananɛnaakɛ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ na ha mɩna'.
46009019	Waʋ mɩ do tɩbɩla fɛʋra wer, sɩ mɩ debire do tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ dee dɩ mɛ̃ ma 'lɛ wɩ waa 'lɛ paar.
46009020	A mɩ hana Juifisɔ, mɩ-n debire dɩ ɩ̃ ho Juifi, dɩ mɛ̃ ma 'lɛ Juifisɔ. A mɩ hana wɩrɛ hanɩ jɔfʋra, mɩ-n debire dɩ ɩ̃ ho jɔfʋ hɩ̃hɩn, sɩrakɛ ga do jɔfʋra mɩ ha ga, dɩ mɛ̃ ma 'lɛ wɩrɛ hanɩ jɔfʋra.
46009021	A mɩ hana jɔfʋ 'leedara, mɩ-n debire dɩ ɩ̃ ho ma hana jɔfʋa', sɩrakɛ ga do mɩ faarɛ Thãgbaa jɔfʋa', sɩ Kirisitn jɔfʋ biro mɩ ha, dɩ mɛ̃ ma 'lɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ jɔfʋa'.
46009022	A mɩ hana yɔyɔa, mɩ-n debire dɩ ɩ̃ ho mɩ yɔɔrɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ ma 'lɛ yɔyɔa; mɩ-n debire dɩ ɩ̃ do thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ, dɩ mɛ̃ ado gɩ ha mɔnakɛ, ma thʋnɛ na taa ɩkhasɔ.
46009023	Tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma-n cʋʋrɔ thɩɛna fɛʋ, dɩ mɛ̃ ma 'lɛrɔ dakha ɩ̃da mer.
46009024	Na jι dιι do wιrɛ n caannι kɔlɔ̃kɔɔ ca paar, fɛʋ n caan, sι tιι bιɛl dιbara n 'lɛ khoraa? Mɛ̃ gι, na-n ca ga 'lɛ'lɛ ca.
46009025	Tibil wo tibilikɛ dɔnι nɔnɔɔ, a-n fʋrɛ dιbara thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra; sι wɛr wι-n cʋʋrɛ wι 'lɛ khor cacadaar dʋʋrra sιι dorakɛ dakʋɛnaa gι, sι se wer, khorιkɛ na dɔnι dakʋɛnaa ga sa 'lɛ.
46009026	Gɛr gι me wer mι-n car, sι ga do baba ga, mι-n thʋrɛ, sι ga do pɔι mι-n ja';
46009027	sι ɩ̃ tomι mι-n ka ma-n ʋʋnnɔ, ma-n cʋgʋʋ a jo, saagado mɛ̃ ga, ma mιιrɛ Thãgbaa thιmιι tιbιlala wer ker na pι, sιι do me wer wι bo mer faa.
46010001	Omιna, mι-n ƴaalɛ na-n dədinə ga, asι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ hale ndɔlɔ̃paarra, dι wɛr fɛʋ kɔɔ kpãsɛrɛ lanyʋɔnna;
46010002	dι wɛr fɛʋ kɔɔ 'lɛr yɔ kpɛɛrɛ ndɔlɔ̃paarra na lanyʋɔnna dιι do awι 'li khara na Mʋιjι gι the;
46010003	dι wɛr fɛʋ kɔɔ khor dιko ca bιɛlιkɛ dɔnι thudaa,
46010004	dι wɛr fɛʋ kɔɔ yɔr thɩ̃ yɔna ca bιɛlιkɛ dɔnι thudaa. Gιdonι wι-n kɔɔ yɔr gιrɛ thɛnι thu boka kɔ̃tιιnaakɛ n kɔɔ kpaan warnι, dι bokaarιlera Kirisiti gι.
46010005	Sι tιbιla bərəəm wɛrra na kɔɔ da Thãgba haarra ga, gιdonι wι kɔɔ thiire le bəənnə.
46010006	Dι ga thɩ̃sɔɔle daan gι do sar thɩ̃ nιrɔrɛ, dι mɛ̃ sa-n do thɩ̃ puu ƴaal thue na-n fʋ sι awι kha ga.
46010007	Na-n debi do thιl jidara, mɔ̃kɛ ιkhasɔ wɛrra kɔɔ hana', mɔ̃kɛ gι kherenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Tιbιlaale kɔɔ toore wι kho wa-n yɔna, sι agιpι wι ιιr wa-n sa bιna.”
46010008	Sa-n do dakha bɔdɛl cʋʋdara mɔ̃kɛ ιkhasɔ wɛrra kɔɔ cʋʋna', dι mɛ̃ tιbιla gbιlanι kpelẽ yẽther kɔɔ ji khiir wi bιɛlla.
46010009	Sa-n fifilə dakha Kɔ̃tιn a na hιιn, mɔ̃kɛ ιkhasɔ wɛrra kɔɔ cʋʋnι dι siisɔ kɔɔ kʋʋr wa'.
46010010	Na-n hũhuun dakha mɔ̃kɛ ιkhasɔ wɛrra n kɔɔ hũhuunni, dι gbõgolõdaar kɔɔ kʋʋr wa'.
46010011	Ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ kɔɔ dã wɛr gι nι sar thɩ̃ɛ, dι wι khere ger ga-n dιιr sι fιlɛ, sɛrɛɛkɛ dananι nɛnɛ̃ pιpιι bɔɔkɛ.
46010012	Gɛr gι dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ n pιɛrnι haar ιnι jιɛ jιιl, n jιι hιιn, a na-n jəə koe.
46010013	Fifiləle na-n dã nι saagado gιrɛ tibil n yιnaa ga; sι Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι sobɔdaar a na tu dι na yι bɩ̃ ber gι jɔ anι fãgara ga, sι fifiləlela a na gbɛbιrɛ the paar dι mɛ̃ na puno na fʋ gar dιbara.
46010014	Gɛr gι nɛrɛɛkɛ mι-n nanι, a nι jι nι fuo hʋnɔnɛ na thιl jir.
46010015	Mι mιιna nɛr mɔ̃kɛ nι donι tιι kpɛsɛsɔ; nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n jʋrɛ gιrɛra mι-n sonι na hιnɛ.
46010016	Bɔ̃bɔna thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ sι-n gbanι dι sa-n khιιna Thãgba, ga do Kirisitira sι bulnə kha ɔɔ tɔmãa? Dι buruukɛ sι-n kuurni, ga do Kirisitira sι bulnə kha ɔɔ tomaa?
46010017	Dι gιdonι buru bιɛl gι-n do, sɛrɛɛkɛ jʋɔnɔnι tomι bιɛl sι do, gιdonι buru bιɛlla sι-n bul kha fɛʋ kho.
46010018	Nι hιnɛ wιrɛ dɔnι Ɩjιrayɛldara tibil yinəna: Wιrɛ n khɔnι bonι ji thɩ̃ɛ, ga do Thãgbara wι bulnə kha mɔ̃ wa-n jiirəəni bonιɛɛle bonι ji paaraa?
46010019	Dι anyera mι-n so thakɛra? A thιɛna gaa, bonι ji nʋʋn dɔ thɩ̃ɛ wɛ? Dι agιbo thιl dɔ thɩ̃ɛ wɛ? Kpei.
46010020	Sι gιrɛ wι-n jinəni bonιɛ, kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔra wι-n ji, ga do Thãgbara ga, dι ma-n ƴaal nι bulo kha na kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔa'.
46010021	Na puno na-n yɔ Kɔ̃tιnι thɩ̃ yɔna, nι bir na-n yɔna kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ thɩ̃ yɔna ga; na puno na bul kha na-n kho Kɔ̃tιnι dιko, sι nι bir na-n khona kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ dιkoa'.
46010022	Gbugi sι-n cʋʋ gι fɔ Kɔ̃tιn yaa? Dι sɛr ba hana fãga a jʋɔ yaa?
46010023	Hʋɛ hale thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ cʋʋra, sι ga do thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ bʋɔnɔa'. Hʋɛ hale thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ cʋʋra, sι ga do thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ n cʋɛ tibil dι khɔ̃ da-n pɛra'.
46010024	Tibil na-n ƴaal thɩ̃ɛ na-n bɔ ιnɛr bιɛlla dιbara ga, sι tιbιla fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl n ka na ƴaalɛ gιrɛ na bɔnι ʋkhara.
46010025	Nʋʋn wo nʋʋnιkɛ wι-n dolonι ƴaa na-n khɔ, sι na-n bule thɩ̃ɛ a gba kpιɛrnɔa';
46010026	gιdonι gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Thιι na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ harɔnι, Kɔ̃tιn hιna.”
46010027	Ado tibilikɛ na dɔnι ha pɛdaara' we nι dιko khʋʋ, dιι da nar dι nι jal, nι khɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wa ha nιnι, sι na-n bule thɩ̃ɛ a gba kpιɛrnɔa'.
46010028	Sι ado tibil so nar aa: Bonιɛ wι jinə; na-n khoa koe, gιdonι ntɛɛle khɛ narnι gɛr dɔ nɔɔ, na kpιɛrnɔɔkɛ ga ιnanι.
46010029	Sι kpιɛrnɔɔkɛ mι sonι, ga do afι thɛthɛɛda mι soa', sι tιι kpιιleeda. Anyeraakɛ tιι kpιι na 'laa na yι dɩɩ ɩ̃ hʋ hanana a na-n so.
46010030	Ado mɩ taa fʋɔr Thãgba sɩ na kho, mɔ̃ ga do wa-n mɩɩ ɩ̃da puu gekɛrara mɩ-n fʋɔrɔnɩ Thãgba?
46010031	Dɩ gɛr gɩ thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nɩ-n khonɩ, agɩbo nɩ-n yɔnɩ, na thɩ̃ doo wo thɩ̃ dookɛ nɩ-n cʋʋnɩ, na-n cʋɛ thɩɛna fɛʋ ga-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i.
46010032	Na-n do nɛ baradaa Juifisɔra, dɩ wɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa wɛ, dɩ Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdarara wa';
46010033	mɔ̃kɛ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n donɩ bʋɔ gɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, dɩ ma da tɩbɩla fɛʋ haar; ma-n ƴaal gɩrɛ na bɔ marna', sɩ gɩrɛ na bɔnɩ tibil jɔjʋɔra dɩ wa 'lɛ taarɛ.
46011001	Nɩ dɔ ɩ̃ phɛldara mɔ̃kɛ mɩ donɩ Kirisitii phɛldaar.
46011002	Mɩ-n khɩɩ nɛr mɔ̃kɛ nɩ-n jɩna mɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, na mɔ̃kɛ nɩ fʋnɩ ɩ̃ so mɔ̃kɛra mɩ kɔɔ mɩɛ nɩnɩ.
46011003	Sɩ mɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɩ jɛ dɩ Kirisiti dɔ yʋʋ konana fɛʋ, sɩ kuun do yʋʋ khɛrra, dɩ Thãgba do yʋʋ Kirisitira.
46011004	Kuun wo kuunikɛ n suboni thɩ̃ɛ da-n bɩɛlna Thãgba, agɩbo Thãgba tukɩrʋ a-n ti, ʋrɛ dʋɔraanɩ yʋʋ a-n beesi.
46011005	Khɛr wo khɛrɩkɛ dakha n bɩɛlnɛnɩ Thãgba, agɩbo Thãgba tukɩrʋ a-n ti na yʋ biire, ʋrɛ dʋɔraanɩ yʋʋ a-n beesi, gɩdonɩ gɩ hʋrɛ yʋʋ a bel.
46011006	Gɩdonɩ a khɛr na kɛɛ thɩ̃ɛ yʋʋra ga, dɔ a khabɩ yʋʋ; dɩ gɩdonɩ yicur thɩ̃ɛ gɩ khɛrra ado a khabɩ yʋʋ, agɩbo ado a bel yʋʋ, dɩ dɔ a na-n kɛɛ thɩ̃ɛ yʋʋra.
46011007	Kuun na teana a na-n kɛa thɩ̃ɛ yʋɔa', gɩdonɩ a-n kuure kha na Thãgba a dona Thãgbaa i dʋbɩdaar, sɩ khɛr or, kuuni i dʋbɩdaar gɩ.
46011008	Gɩdonɩ ga do khɛrɩ pa Thãgba ti kuuna', sɩ kuuni pa a ti khɛr.
46011009	Dɩ ga do khɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ Thãgba tiro kuuna', sɩ kuun dɔ nɔɔ dɩ tiro khɛr.
46011010	Gɛr gɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ khɛr teena a hanana thɩ̃ɛ yʋɔ, gɩ nɩna dɩ bɩɛl hale a hananaa hʋɛ.
46011011	Sɩ wo Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɛthɛra, khɛr na hale a kuun na halaa ga, dɩ kuun na hale a khɛr na halaa ga.
46011012	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ khɛr thenɩ kuunna, ɔmɛ̃ khɛr do nɔɔ dɩ kuun hale, sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ Thãgbara gɩ the.
46011013	Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n ka jʋrɛ hɩnɛ, gɩ teere kha khɛr na-n bɩɛl Thãgba na yʋ biire ya?
46011014	Ne wer na yɩɛrakɛ dɩɩ do ado kuun hana yʋsuune vʋɔlvʋɔl, yicuru gɩ-n dʋʋraa;
46011015	sɩ ado khɛr or hana gɩ dɩɩ dʋʋraa i dʋbɩdaa gaa? Gɩdonɩ Thãgba haarɛ yʋsuune vʋɔlvʋɔl gɩ dʋɔraa kɛɛdaa.
46011016	Ado gɩ da tibillə dɩ na bana, sɛrɛ sa mɩlna thɩ̃ɛ thaka', dɩ Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdara gɩrakɛ dakha ga.
46011017	Mɩ ha nɛr thɩmɩɩ nɔ ʋrɛ wer, sɩ gɩrɛraakɛ ma punoni na khɩɩ na' dʋɔn gɩdonɩ, na-n gbɛbɩ kha gɩ ka cʋɛ nɩ nɩ bɔr na-n pɛra', sɩɩ do nɩ ka puurore dɩ na-n pɛr.
46011018	Caca thɩ̃ɛ, mɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n gbɛbɩnɩ kha mɔ̃kɛ nɩ donɩ we gbɛbɩdara, leere n har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ mɩ pɛ gɛr haar kho bɩɛl.
46011019	Gɩdonɩ dɔ thʋ̃ kha wer n ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ mɛ̃ wa jɩ wɩrɛ dɔnι sobɔdara anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
46011020	Wo, ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n gbɛbɩnɩ kha pa bɩɛl, ga do Kɔ̃tɩnɩ dɩko nɩ-n khoa'.
46011021	Gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ na-n khonɩ dɩkɔra, tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl n kɔɔ mar dɩ wa-n kho awɩ thɛthɛɛ dɩko, sɩ ʋ n toona kɔmɛr, dɩ taan na-n kʋ ʋ.
46011022	Na hana cɔna ka na khonɩ na-n yɔna gaa? Dɩ agɩbo Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdara nɩ-n beesi na-n pɛna wɩrɛ na hananɩ thɩ̃a' yicuru ya? Anye ma thʋ̃ na so nar? Ɩ̃ khɩa nɩ wɛ? Ma khɩɩ nι gelelaale wera'.
46011023	Gιdonι Kɔ̃tιnι pa mι kɔɔ 'lɛ gιrɛɛkɛ mι kɔɔ dιιr nιnι, gι sor ayι: Dιtιnɔɔkɛ wι kɔɔ liirnanι Jeju Kɔ̃tιn, a kɔɔ gbaar buru,
46011024	dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ fʋɔrnι Thãgba a pɛr pι, a kuure sa so ayι: “Gιrɛ dɔ ɩ̃ tomιιkɛ cʋɔrɛnι anι sora; na-n cʋɛ thakɛ a na jɛna mι.”
46011025	Dι mɔ̃ wι khonι na pι, a gbaar thɩ̃ yɔnanɛ oti a so ayι: “Thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ dʋɔn nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛ phaakɛ thɛnι ɩ̃ tɔmιna; na-n cʋɛ thakɛ a na jɛna mι bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ na-n yɔ gιnι.”
46011026	Gιdonι bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ nι-n khonι buruukɛ, dι na-n yɔna thɩ̃ yɔnanɛɛkɛ, Kɔ̃tιnι khi nι-n nιna phaphapha a ιna.
46011027	Gɛr gι ʋrɛɛkɛ na khɔnι buruukɛ a na yɔna Kɔ̃tιnι thɩ̃ yɔnaakɛ na fιlɛɛkɛ na teanι kha ga, a na 'lɛr sor Kɔ̃tιnι tomιra na Kɔ̃tιnι tɔmιna.
46011028	Gɛr gι dɔ tibil n bəər ɔɔ bɩ̃ a hιιn, sι a kho buru a yɔna thɩ̃ yɔnanɛ.
46011029	Gιdonι ʋrɛɛkɛ khɔnι a yɔna sι aa jι dιι do Kɔ̃tιnι tomι ga, kιιlʋ a kho, a yɔna kιιlʋ a pɛr dιbara.
46011030	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dι tomι sιdara na khodara jɔr anι thɩ̃thιιn, dι tibil jɔjʋɔ na-n khiir.
46011031	Sι ado sι bəər asι bɩ̃ na hιιn, sa 'lɛ kιιlʋa'.
46011032	Sι ɔbɔɔkɛ sι-n 'lɛnι kɩɩlʋ, Kɔ̃tιn n naarɛ sι, dι mɛ̃ sa 'lɛ so heene nakha thιdara ga.
46011033	Mɛ̃ gι ɩ̃ omisɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n gbɛbιnι kha nι kho dιkɔ, nι jιlɛ na pιɛrɛ kha.
46011034	Ado kɔmɛr fʋrɛ ntɛ a kɔɔ khɔ dιkor ɔɔ cɔ, dι mɛ̃ na gbɛbι kha na-n pɛ kιιlʋ dιbara ga. A mι pɔ, gɛr ma gbɛbιrɔ yɛ̃ thɩ̃sɔ.
46012001	Sɩ omɩna, ado gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Thu Phuu khaardasɔ gɩ, ge wer ma-n ƴaal na-n jɩ mɔ̃ gɩ hanaa ga.
46012002	Nɩ jɩrɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ donɩ thɩldara, wɩ-n kɔɔ haal nɛr dɩ na-n kpaan ba, thɩlalaakɛ na-n punoneni na mɩɩ nʋɔa'.
46012003	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ma-n so nar gɩrɛ ayɩ: Tibilikɛ na sɔnɩ nayɩ, ɩnɩ sʋɔn Jeju, ga do Thãgbaa Thurə gɩ tha'; dɩ tibil na puno na so nayɩ: Jeju dɔ Kɔ̃tɩn, saagado Thu Phuurə gɩ thaa ga.
46012004	Khaarda caar dɩɩdɩɩ hale, sɩ Thu Phuu bɩɛllala gɩ the.
46012005	Bul thɔ̃ caar dɩɩdɩɩ hale, sɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛllala gɩ the.
46012006	Thɩ̃ cʋʋ caar dιιdιι hale, sι Thãgba bιɛlla gιιkɛ n cʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋle dι ga-n dã tιbιlala fɛʋ.
46012007	Tιbιla fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl n 'lɛr Thu Phuurə thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ, ga-n bul tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
46012008	Ʋkha n 'lɛr kpɛsɛ thιmιιr, dιι the Thu Phuurə, ʋkha n 'lɛr jι thιmιιr, dιι the Thu Phuu bιɛllala.
46012009	Ʋkha n 'lɛr ha pɛrɛ, dιɩ the Thu Phuu bιɛllala, ʋkha n 'lɛr kho kpɛɛ khaardaa, dιι the Thu Phuu bιɛllala.
46012010	Ʋkha n 'lɛr punone da-n cʋʋna nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ; ʋkha n 'lɛr Thãgba tukιr tir; ʋkha n 'lɛr jιιr da-n jιna gιrɛ thɛnι Thu Phuurə na gιrɛ na thɛnι Thu Phuurə ga; ʋkha n 'lɛr thιmιι kpιι mιιrɛ dιιdιι; ʋkha n 'lɛr punone da-n finə thιmιι kpιιkɛ n mιanι.
46012011	Thu Phuu bιɛlla gι 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽekɛ n cʋɛnι ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛra fɛʋ, da-n tιnɛ tιbιla fɛʋ dιιdιι mɔ̃kɛ a-n ƴaalnι.
46012012	Gιdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ tomɩr donɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛl sa hana ɓaanʋ dɩɩ jɔr, dɩ mɔ̃kɛ tomɩ ɓaanʋsɔɔle jɔrnɩnakɛ sɩ tomɩ bɩɛlla gɩ do, mɛ̃ gɩ ha na Kirisiti.
46012013	A Juifisɔ ha sɩ, a wɩrɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa wɛ, a dea wɛ, a waɩa wɛ, Thu Phuurəəkɛ dɔnɩ bɩɛl wɩ kɔɔ kpɛɛ sɛrɛ fɛʋ, sɩ debiro sɩ do tomɩ bɩɛl, dɩ sɛrɛ fɛʋ Thu Phuu bɩɛl sɩ kɔɔ yɔ.
46012014	Gɛr gɩ tomɩr na do ɓã bɩɛla', sɩ ɓaanʋ jɔrɛ.
46012015	Ado nɔɔ sor ayɩ, gɩdonɩ ɩna do nyɔ̃a', ɩna do tomɩrɩda ga, gelelakɛ na cʋgʋʋrɛ da do tomɩrɩda geraa ya?
46012016	Dɩ ado nũu sor ayɩ, gɩdonɩ ɩna do yirə', ɩna do tomɩrɩda ga, gelelakɛ na cʋgʋʋrɛ da do tomɩrɩda geraa ya?
46012017	Ado yire tomɩr do fɛʋ, sɩ nɩdaa kana ga ha? Ado nɩdaa tomɩr do fɛʋ, sɩ hʋ̃ nɩdaa kana ga ha?
46012018	Mee Thãgba pɩɛr tomι ɓaanʋsɔ bɩɛlbɩɛl tomɩrra mɔ̃kɛ a-n ƴaalnɩ.
46012019	Dɩ ado fɛʋ dor tomɩ ɓã bɩɛl, sɩ kana tomɩr na ha?
46012020	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ dɩ tomɩ ɓaanʋ jɔr, sɩ dɩ tomɩr do bɩɛl dɩbara.
46012021	Yire na puno na so nyɔɔna nayɩ, ɩna hana ɔɔ ƴaalaa ga; dɩ yʋʋ gɩ a na so nɛɛra nayɩ, ɩna hana awɩ ƴaalaa ga.
46012022	Sɩ tomɩ ɓã ƴɩrɛ n kanɩ ho sar wa hana fãga jɔjɔa', sɩ thɩ̃ɛ gɩɩkɛ teananɩ hananɛ.
46012023	Tomɩ ɓaanʋsɔɔkɛ sa-n jɩɩnɩ therna bɔɔbɔa', sɩ-n jɩɛ cʋ gɩ jɔɔ; mɛ̃ asɩ tomɩ ɓãsɔɔkɛ na bʋɔnɔnɩ yɩra' n ka 'lɛ cʋrɛ jɔɔ dɩ a-n kar.
46012024	Sɩ gɩrɛ kanɩ bɔr yɩr na-n 'lɛ mã'. Sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ gbɛbɩrɛ tomɩr a gba cʋʋr a pɛr tomɩ ɓaanaakɛ na jɩɛnɩ 'lɛ cʋʋra',
46012025	dɩ mɛ̃ leere na hale tomtrra ga, sɩ gɩ do mɛ̃ tomɩ ɓaanʋsɔ n jɩɩ hɩɩn kha na fɩl bɩɛl.
46012026	Dɩ ado tomɩ ɓã bɩɛl na gaar bʋɔ, tomɩ ɓaanʋ fɛʋ n gaarɛ kha na ɔr, a wɩ cʋ tomɩ ɓã bɩɛl, tomɩ ɓaanʋsɔ fɛʋ n kãkarɛ kha na ɔr.
46012027	Nɛr dɔ Kirisitii tomɩ, dɩ nɛr dɔ ɔɔ tomɩ ɓãsɔ dɩɩdɩɩ.
46012028	Dɩ Thãgba pɛrɛ we gbɛbɩdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn: Cacara, thɔ̃thɔna; balanyɔ, Thãgba tukɩr tidara; balãther, dɩɩrdara; agɩpɩ, nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ cʋʋdara; agɩpɩ, wɩrɛ hananɩ kho kpɛɛ khaardaa, na bubulo, na ƴɛ kʋla, na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ dɩɩdɩɩ mɩɩdara.
46012029	Fɛʋ n dɔ thɔ̃thɔna kã? Fɛʋ n dɔ Thãgba tukɩr tidara kã? Dɩ fɛʋ n dɔ dɩɩrdara kã? Dɩ fɛʋ n cʋɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ kã?
46012030	Dɩ fɛʋ n hana kho kpɛɛ khaardaa kã? Dɩ fɛʋ n mɩa thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ kã? Dɩ fɛʋ n fien thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ kã?
46012031	Na-n hanana khaardaasɔɔkɛ baannɩɩ ƴaal; sɩ ma nɩ narɛ hʋɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnɩnakɛ a ka.
46013001	A mɩ jɩ tibil caar fɛʋʋ thɩmɩɩ na mɩɩ, a gɩrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ n mɩɩnɩ gɩ, sɩ a ma hana naʋa', nʋɔ mɩ-n kɩɛr oro oro gbõgbõ khaa, agɩbo dẽgelẽbi khaa wele wele.
46013002	A mɩ hana punone a na tinə Thãgba tukɩrʋ, a mɩ jɩrɛrakɛ dakha thɩ̃ gbulsɔ fɛʋ, a hanana jɩɩr ɓibi, ado mɩ hananakɛ ha pɛrɛ ɓibiikɛ na əəleni gɔ̃gɔna, sɩ a ma hana naʋa', ma do thɩ̃a'.
46013003	A mɩ gbarakɛ ɩ̃ thɩ̃ fɛʋ a tɩnɛ bɔdara, a ɩ̃ tomɩ mɩ gbarakɛ 'laa wɩ thiə, sɩ a ma hana naʋa', gele na taa mɩ bʋɔa'.
46013004	Naʋ n hananɛ ha fʋrɛ, naʋ n bulole haar ka, naʋ na-n gbugə', naʋ na-n nɩna dɩbara ga, aa-n ka irə',
46013005	naʋ na-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na teanɩ kha gaaga, aa-n yɩrna ɔɔda ga, aa-n hana nĩkhiə', aa-n therna puureekɛ wɩ-n cʋgʋʋna';
46013006	gɩrɛ na sarana' na-n daaraa ga, sɩ sobɔr n daaraa.
46013007	Naʋ na-n bo da-n ɩɩ haanɩ dɩ para ga, a-n hananɛ ha pɛrɛ thɩɛna fɛʋ, a-n hananɛ nũ pɛrɛ thɩɛna fɛʋ, a-n hananɛ ha fʋrɛ thɩɛna fɛʋ.
46013008	Naʋ na hana khu paara'. Thãgba tukɩr tir na phor na ka, thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ mɩɩrɛ ga pɩrrɛ, jɩɩr na phor na ka;
46013009	gɩdonɩ jɩ kuru sɩ hana, dɩ Thãgba tukɩr kuru sɩ-n ti.
46013010	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ thʋnanɩ bɔr ka na ɩnɩ, gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dakuru na phor na ka.
46013011	Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ donɩ bɩsaan, bɩsaanɛ mɩ-n mɩɩ, dɩ bɩsaanɛ mɩ-n kpɩɛr, dɩ mɔ̃ mɩ-n kuurni na bɩnɛ, bɩsã khaara gɩ oti. Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ khɔnɩ pɩ, gɩrɛ dɔnɩ bɩsaanɛ pho marɛ ka.
46013012	Nĩkɛ sɩ-n yɩrɛ ɩhĩɛ mɔ tibil n yɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ hɩɩnʋna, sɩ biroo sɩ-n yɩɛ, sɩ a bɔɔ dã gbelẽ gbelẽ sa yɩɛ. Nĩkɛ dakuru sɩ jɩ, sɩ a bɔɔ dã ma jɩ gɛr vʋ̃ʋ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba jɩ mɩnɩ.
46013013	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ, thɩ̃ɛ yẽtherɩkɛ jɩlɛnɩ dʋɔn: Ha pɛrɛ, nũ pɛrɛ, naʋ, sɩ geleelerarakɛ dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ jɔnɩ fɛʋ dʋɔn naʋra.
46014001	Na-n gbuoro naʋ ƴaalɛ yʋʋ; sɩ na-n ƴaalɛ dakha Thu Phuu khaardasɔ, sɩ gɩrɛ na jɩɩnɩ ƴaallakɛ jɔɔ dʋɔn Thãgba tukɩr tir.
46014002	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ n mɩanɩ thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, ga do tɩbɩla a-n mɩɩna ga, sɩ Thãgba a-n mɩɩna. Gɩdonɩ tibil na-n jɩ gɩrɛ a-n sona', sɩ Thu Phuu n cʋgɛɛ da-n mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ gbul.
46014003	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n tenɩ Thãgba tukɩrʋ, tɩbɩla a-n ka da-n mɩɩna gɩ cʋʋ wɩ wɩ hana khɔ̃ pɛrɛ, na ƴɛ kʋʋl jaal, na ha faarɛ.
46014004	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n mιanι thιmιιr na thιmιι kpιι ɔɔ thɛthɛ gι-n cʋʋ da-n khɔ̃, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n tenɩ Thãgba tukɩrʋ, we gbɛbɩdara a-n cʋʋ dɩ wa-n khɔ̃.
46014005	Mɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ na-n mɩa thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, sɩ ƴaal kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ mɩ hananɩnakɛ jɔɔ dʋɔn, na-n te Thãgba tukɩrʋ. Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ n tenɩ Thãgba tukɩrʋ, a kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ ʋrɛ n mɩanɩ thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, agado ɔɔ thɩmɩɩra a-n fi dɩ we gbɛbɩdara na-n 'lɛrɔ khɔ̃ pɛra'.
46014006	Sɩ omɩna nɩ hɩnɛ, anyee bɔ ca ga taa nɩ, ado mɩ pɔ anɩ pa, a na mɩɩ thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, agado thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ, na jɩɩr, na Thãgba tukɩr tir, na dɩɩrɛ mɩ-n mɩɩna na?
46014007	Thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na hananɩnakɛ yirə', sɩ gɩ hananɛ wire, a bɩɩl gɩ, a salãa gɩ, ado bɩɩl na-n ʋ̃ dɩɩ yɩra', mɔ̃ wa jɩ gɩrɛ gɩ-n sonɩ? Ado salãa na-n bɩ̃ dιι yιra', mɔ̃ wa jι gιrɛ gι-n sonι?
46014008	Dι dakha ado wa jιɩ ʋ̃ tutuə', ʋmɔ̃ na gbɛbɩrɛ ko ke gbɛbɩrʋʋ?
46014009	Mɛ̃ gɩ, nɛrɛ dakha, ado anɩ delẽbi thɩmɩɩ na-n yɩr casa', mɔ̃ tibil na fʋ sɩ na jɩ gɩrɛ n mɩanɩ? Gɩdonɩ bʋla bʋla nɩ-n mɩɩ.
46014010	Thɩmɩɩ caar dɩɩdɩɩ na jɔr thɩɩra kpãkpalã ga, sɩ thɩmɩɩr na hale sa 'lee kɩrʋa'.
46014011	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ado ma jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ tibil n mɩɩna', kpakpal ma do okɛrara n mɩanɩ, dɩ ɔr dakha na do marɛ kpakpal.
46014012	Mɛ̃ gɩ, nɛrɛ dakha, mɔ̃kɛ na hananɩ Thu Phuu khaarda ƴaalɛ kpãkpalã ga, na-n ƴaalɛ a 'lɛ jɔɔ gɩrɛɛkɛ na cʋɛnɩ we gbɛbɩdara dɩ wa khɔ̃ wa-n pɛr.
46014013	Gɛr gɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n mɩanɩ thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, dɔ a bɩɛl Thãgba a haa thɩmɩɩ fiir.
46014014	Gɩdonɩ a ma bɩɛl Thãgba na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, ɩ̃ thu n bɩɛlnɛ, sɩ ɩ̃ kpɩɛr wer kpalalɛ too.
46014015	Dɩ mɔ̃ ga ha? Ma bɩɛlɛ Thãgba gɩ the thuerə, sɩ dakha ma bɩɛlɛ Thãgba gɩ the kpɩɛrɛra. Ma khɩnɛ nɩɛ gɩ the thuerə, sɩ dakha ma khɩnɛ nɩɛ gɩ the kpɩɛrɛra.
46014016	A fa fʋɔr Thãgba dɩɩ do thuerə gɩ-n the, mɔ̃ ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ nũpɛthe na fʋ sɩ na dee “Amɛn” afɩ Thãgba fʋɔrra, aa jɩnɩ gɩrɛ fɩ-n sona?
46014017	Fɩ-n fʋɔrɛ Thãgba wer na sobɔr, sɩ ga cʋʋ tɩɩ kpɩɩ da khɔ̃ na pɛra'.
46014018	Mɩ-n khɩɩrɛ Thãgba gɩrɛraakɛ mɩ-n mɩɩnɩ thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ dɩ ɩ̃ jɔ nɩ fɛʋ.
46014019	Sɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn, mɩ nar ɩ̃ mɩa thɩmɩɩ be yemɔɩ, sɩ gɩ do kpɩɛrɛra gɩ the, gɩ dɩɩr ɩkhasɔ, gɩ baar thɩmɩɩ be gbɩlanɩ yʋɔrɩkɛ ma mɩɩnɩ na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ.
46014020	Omɩna wei, na-n do bɩsana bɩ̃ kuurera gaa koe. Sɩ puu cʋʋrɛra wer, nɩ dɔ bɩsã bii, sɩ ado bɩ̃ kuurdaara gɩ, nɩ dɔ kũu bɩ̃ cɩɩsɔ.
46014021	Gɩ kherere Thãgbaa jɔfʋra ayɩ: “Kɔ̃tɩn sor ayɩwɔɔ: Ca kpɩɩsɔ na kpakpalaa nɔ ma gba na mɩɩna na mɩɩmɩɩ wa tibilsɔraakɛ, sɩrakɛ wa pɛ mɩ nũə'.”
46014022	Gɛr hɩna, jɩɩn thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ mɩɩrɛ do, ga do wɩrɛraakɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar ga, sɩ wɩrɛraakɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haara'. Sɩ Thãgba tukɩr tir do jɩɩn, ga do wɩrɛraakɛ na pɩɛrnɩ haaraa ga, sɩ ha pɛdarara.
46014023	Dɩ a mɛ̃ gɩ, a we gbɛbɩdaar haar gbɛbɩ kha, dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na mɩɩ thɩmɩɩr na thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ, dɩ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ nũpɛthesɔ, agɩbo wɩrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ ha pɛdara ga, lõ le, ga do wa sor nayɩ yʋ budara hanaa?
46014024	Sɩ ado tɩbɩla fɛʋ na ti Thãgba tukɩrʋ, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ ha pɛdaara', agɩbo nũpɛthe, lõ le, tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ thɩmɩɩ na punoone, dɩ a na 'laarɛ dakha na yɩ mɔ̃kɛ a hanɩ;
46014025	dɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ keranɩ ɔɔ hara ga yɩrrɛ, dɩ a na jire na sumo a na-n fʋɔr Thãgba sa a so ayɩ: “Thãgba har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn ger.”
46014026	Omɩna, dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ teena gɩ hana? Ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ-n gbɛbɩnɩ kha dɩ ʋkha nɛrɛra n hana nɩɛ, ʋ n hana dɩɩrɛ, ʋ n hana nɩrɔ thɩmɩɩr, ʋ n hana thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ mɩɩrɛ, ʋ n hana thɩmɩɩ fiir, dɔ na-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ we gbɛbɩdara n khɔ̃ wa-n pɛr.
46014027	Ado thɩmɩɩ kpɩɩ mɩɩdara hale, wɩ dɔ tɩbɩla yenyɔ agɩbo yẽther dɩbara, sɩ wa-n mɩa kpa kha kpa kha, dɩ dɔ thɩmɩɩ fidaar n hale a na-n fi.
46014028	Sι ado thιmιι fidaar na hala', ntɛ n pιra pɔbι we gbɛbιdaraa thɩ̃thιιn, sι na mιa dɩbara nakha Thãgba.
46014029	Sɩ ado wɩrɛ n tenɩ Thãgba tukɩrʋ gɩ, dɔ yenyɔ agɩbo yẽther na-n mɩɩ, sɩ wɩrɛ sɛnɩ n jʋrɛ gɩrɛra n mɩanɩ na hɩnɛ.
46014030	Sɩ ado tibil kpɩɩkɛ tɔɔnɩ hananɛ nɩrɔ thɩmɩɩr, dɔ cacadaar n pɩr.
46014031	Gɩdonɩ nɩ punone fɛʋ a ti Thãgba tukɩrʋ kpa kha kpa kha, dɩ mɛ̃ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na 'lɛr dɩɩrɛ, fɛʋ n 'lɛ dakha ha faarɛ.
46014032	Gɩrɛ Thãgbaa Thu n cʋʋnɩ Thãgba tukɩr tidara dɩ wa-n mɩɩ, gɩ-n wurre Thãgba tukιr tidarara.
46014033	Gιdonι Thãgba na do bʋla bʋla Thãgba ga, sι ha ie Thãgba a do. Mɔ̃kɛ gι-n hanι paar fɛʋʋkɛ tɩɩ phuusɔ n gbɛbɩnɩ kha,
46014034	dɔ khɛra n pɩr pɔbɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa pa, gɩdonɩ wa hana hʋɛ na mɩɩ thɩmɩɩra', sɩ wɩ jɔ dɩbara mɔ̃kɛ dakha Thãgbaa jɔfʋ sonɩ.
46014035	Ado wɩ-n ƴaalɛ wɩ jɩ thɩ̃ɛ, wa-n bulene awɩ kosɔ le cʋɔrɔ, gιdonι ƴicur thɩ̃ɛ gι, a khɛr na mιι thɩ̃ɛ we gbɛbιdaraa pa.
46014036	Anι pa Thãgbaa thιmιι ba therakɛ yaa, dι agιbo nɛr dιbara gι ba dã yaa?
46014037	Ado tibil pɛr haar Thãgba tukιr tidaar ha nι, agιbo Thu Phuudaar ha nι, dɔ ntɛ n tu dakha dι gιrɛ mι khere narnι Kɔ̃tιnι jɔfʋ gι do.
46014038	Dι ado ntɛ yι ιnι-n bor, a bɔ bɛɛ.
46014039	Gɛr gι ɩ̃ omisɔ, na-n ƴaalɛ na haar fɛʋ Thãgba tukιr tir, sι na-n pιɛr tibil a na-n mιι thιmιιr na thιmιι kpιaa ga.
46014040	Dɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na-n cʋʋ na fιl bʋɔ, dι dakha nyanyaanɛ na-n hala'.
46015001	Omιna, mι cʋʋ nɛr nɩ jɛna tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ dakha a jɩɩllɔ kɩbɩ.
46015002	Gɛr dɔ dakha gɩrɛ dɔnɩ nɔɔ dɩ nɩ 'lɛrɔ taarɛ, ado nɩ fʋ gɛr gel mɔ̃kɛ mɩ kɔɔ mɩι nιnι; ado mɛ̃ gι yuuə', ga dor mɔlɔ nι kɔɔ pɛr haar.
46015003	Caca thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ιkɛ mι kɔɔ dιιr nιnι, kɛ dɔnι dakha gιrɛ mι kɔɔ 'lɛnι dʋɔn: Kirisiti kɔɔ khire asι sopugosɔra mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonι,
46015004	dι wι kɔɔ dʋʋrɛ, sɩ a ɩɩrɛ a the khirera balãther wirera, mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ,
46015005	dɩ a kɔɔ nɩnanɛ ɔɔbara Sefasɩ agɩpɩ yʋɔr yenyɔra.
46015006	Agɩpɩ a kɔɔ nɩnanɛ ɔɔbara bɔ bɩɛlla omɩna taamɔɩra na dɛbɩrɛ, kɛ jɔɔ hanɩkɛ nĩ na yire, sɩ dɩ ɩkhasɔ daar daanɩkɛ dɔnɩ khir.
46015007	Agɩpɩ a nɩnanɛ ɔɔbara Jakɩ, agɩpɩ dɩ nɩna ɔɔbara wo thɔ̃thɔnana fɛʋ.
46015008	Agɩpɩ fɛʋ a nɩna mɛr dakha ɔɔbara, sιrakɛ mɛr hʋɔn ʋrɛɛkɛ wɩ ɓɔrnɩ kɔ̃.
46015009	Gɩdonɩ mɛr dɔ dabuu fɩɩʋ thɔ̃thɔnasɔra, ma teena wɩ we mɩ thɔ̃thɔna', gɩdonɩ mɩ kɔɔ kpoore Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdarasɔra.
46015010	Sɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ do gɩrɛ mɩ donɩ gɩrɛ, dɩ ɔɔ bɔ jɩra mɛrɛra na kɔɔ do mɔlɔ kpɩɩraka', sɩ mɩ-n ka dor thɔma a jɔ wɛr fɛʋ, sɩrakɛ ga do ɩ̃ pa gɩ thaa koe, sɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩɩkɛ a kɔɔ jɩ mɩnɩ bʋɔra dɔ nɔɔ.
46015011	Gɛr gɩ ado mɛr gɩ ado wɛr gɩ, gɛr dɔ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩkɛ sɩ-n mɩɩnɩ, dɩ gɛrra nɩ kɔɔ pɛr haar.
46015012	Dɩ ado Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ n mɩɩrɛ ayɩ: Kirisiti kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a the khirera, dɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ sɩ ɩkhasɔ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn n yɩ: Khi ɩɩrɛ na hala?
46015013	Ado khi ɩɩrɛ na-n hala', Kirisiti dakha na kɔɔ ɩɩr na the khirera ga.
46015014	Dɩ ado Kirisiti na kɔɔ ɩɩr a the khirera ga, ga dor Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩkɛ sɩ-n mɩɩnɩ mɔlɔ gɩ, dɩ anɩ ha pɛ dakha mɔlɔ gɩ.
46015015	Dɩ ga dorakɛ sõso so jɩdara sɩ do Thãgbara, gɩdonɩ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩrɛ a pɛr Thãgbara ayɩ, a kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ Kirisiti dɩ the khirera, sɩɩ do aa kɔɔ ɩɩrʋʋ dɩ the khirera ga, dɩ gɩdonɩ khe na-n ɩɩr ger dɩ wɩ the khirera ga.
46015016	Gɩdonɩ ado khe na ɩɩr na the khirera ga, Kirisiti dakha na kɔɔ ɩɩr na the khirera ga.
46015017	Dɩ ado Kirisiti na kɔɔ ɩɩr a the khirera ga, anɩ ha pɛ mɔlɔ gɩ do, ga dor nɩ hale anɩ sopugosɔra 'lo;
46015018	dɩ ga dor dakha wɩrɛ pɛnɩ Kirisiti haar sa daar daanɩkɛ dɔnɩ khir wɩ buure.
46015019	Ado ga yi hanaakɛ thɩɩra dɩbara sɩ yɩrɔ nũ pɛrɛ sɩ hana Kirisitira, ga dor sɛr n kɔ bʋɔ a jɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
46015020	Sɩ gel Kirisiti kɔɔ ɩɩr a the khirera, ɔr dɔ cacadaar wɩrɛraakɛ daarɛnɩ daanɩkɛ dɔnɩ khir.
46015021	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ khir thenɩ tɩɩ bɩɛlla, mɛ̃ dakha khi ɩɩrɛ the tɩɩ bɩɛlla.
46015022	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ Adã donɩ nɔɔ dɩ fɛʋ na-n khiir, mɛ̃ dakha Kirisiti na do nɔɔ dɩ fɛʋ na bir na 'lɛ yire;
46015023	sɩ jɔ kha jɔ kha gɩ, Kirisiti n do cacadaar, agɩpɩ ɔɔ bir ɩ̃ bɔɔ, wɩrɛɛkɛ Kirisitira hɩnɩ.
46015024	Agɩpɩ khu paar n dã dɩphã, liir a na gba fãgadaar dʋʋr na ha Thãgba Thɩrɛ, ɔbɔɔkɛ a na bũburoni dakpɛna yʋʋsɔ fɛʋ, na hʋ hanadara fɛʋ, na fãgadara fɛʋ na pɩ.
46015025	Gɩdonɩ dɔ a do fãgadaar phaphapha a jəəro ɔɔ lãlaardara fɛʋ nɛɛ.
46015026	Pɩpɩɩ lãlaardaarɩkɛ na bũburoneni khir gɩ,
46015027	gɩdonɩ “Thãgba gbaar thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ jəəro nɛɛ.” Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ ayɩ, thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ jʋʋraarɛ, gɩ yɩrrɛ mɛ̃ dɩ ʋrɛra pɩɛrnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ jəəro nɛɛ, ɔr dɩbara sɛ.
46015028	Ɔbɔɔkɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na jʋʋraanɩ na pɩ, le Bikuuni thɛthɛ na jo dɩbara ʋrɛraakɛra cʋɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ jʋʋraa, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgba na do yʋʋ fɛʋra ɓibi.
46015029	Dɩ ado ga ha thala', anye wɩrɛ wɩ kpɛɛnɩ nyʋɔnɔ kherə na yɩ? Dɩ adorakɛ khe na ɩɩr khirera kpɩɩa', mɔ̃ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ wa kpɛɛ wɩ nyʋɔnɔ kherə?
46015030	Dɩ sɛrɛ dakha, anyera sɩ-n faa dɩbara bɔ kʋrra bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛra?
46015031	Sobɔr gɩ omɩna, mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ ɩ̃ məbida asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira waa gel, mɛna gɩ ha na gɩrɛ, wire fɛʋ khikhi togʋʋ mɩ-n too.
46015032	Ado mɔ̃kɛ tibil kpɩɛrɛ hanɩ mɩ kɔɔ kɛ̃kɛrɛna hɔ̃ nɛbi kho thɩ̃ɛ Efɛjɩ dɩɩra, sɩɩ do khe na ɩɩr na the khirera ga, anyee kho ca ma 'lɛ gelela? Dɩ sa-n cʋɛ gɩrɛ sokpaa sɔnɩ ger bɛɛ: “Sɩ khɔɔ a na yɔna, gɩdonɩ cʋɔ sa khiire.”
46015033	Na-n fɩɩl anɩbara ga: Tɩɩ puu kuune 'lã'lã'lã n kʋɛrɛ fɩl bʋɔ.
46015034	Nɩ dɔ gɩ gba nɩ khər mɔ̃kɛ gɩ teenɩ kha, dɩ na-n cʋʋ sopugoə', gɩdonɩ ɩkhasɔ na jɩ Thãgba ga. Mɩ sor thakɛ yicuru n fɔ nɩ.
46015035	Sɩ ʋkha na sor: Mɔ̃ khe na fʋ sɩ na ɩɩr na the khirera? Anyee tomɩ ca wa bir na ɩna gɩrɛ kper?
46015036	Də̃bəəlu ha fɩ bã; gɩrɛ fɩ-n diirni na hana yire saagado gɩ kɔɔ khire ɓoaa ga.
46015037	Ɔbɔɔkɛ fa-n diirni, ga do phuloleekɛ na phonɩ fɩ-n kɔɔ gba diirə', sɩ bire gɩ, agado jʋ birə' dɩɩ do thɩ̃ diir kpɩɩ.
46015038	Sɩ Thãgba n 'laaraa tomɩr mɔ̃kɛra a kɔɔ ƴaalnɩnakɛ gɩ hana, dɩ a-n har thɩ̃ diire bɩɛlbɩɛl tomɩr dɩɩdɩɩ.
46015039	Nʋʋn fɛʋ na-n do nʋ̃ ca bɩɛla', tibildaa n har kpɩɩ, dɩ nʋmaada n ha kpɩɩ, dɩ 'lominəəda n ha kpɩɩ, dɩ thʋmaada n ha kpɩɩ.
46015040	Yu thɩ̃ɛsɔ n hale, thɩdaasɔ n hale, sɩ ƴũ thɩ̃ɛɛ carã pa n har kpɩɩ, dɩ thɩdaa n ha kpɩɩ ga ƴɛra.
46015041	Wiree carã n har kpɩɩ, dɩ porɩ carã n ha kpɩɩ, dɩ ƴepələ̃bee carã n ha kpɩɩ, gɩdonɩ ƴepələ̃berarakɛ bɩɛlɩ carã n har kpɩɩ na ʋ̃ ƴepələ̃bi.
46015042	Mɛ̃ gɩ ha khee ɩɩrra, tomɩ kʋɛnaa wɩ-n dʋ mɔ̃ wɩ-n diirni thɩ̃ɛ, sɩ mɔ̃ a-n ɩɩrnɩ aa-n do dakʋɛnaa ga.
46015043	Mɔ̃ wa-n dʋʋnι dabeesinaa a-n do, sι mɔ̃ a-n ιιrnι cʋrɛ a-n ιιrna. Mɔ̃ wa-n dʋʋnɩ dayɔgɔ a-n do, sɩ mɔ̃ a-n ɩɩrnɩ fãga haar a-n do.
46015044	Mɔ̃ wa-n dʋʋnɩ tomɩ jaar a-n do, sɩ mɔ̃ a-n ɩɩrnɩ thudaa a-n do; tomɩ jaar n hale, dɩ thudaa n hale dakha.
46015045	Gɛr gɩ dɩɩ khere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra dakha ayɩ: “Caca tibilikɛ dɔnɩ Adã debire a do tibilikɛ hananɩ yire”, sɩ pɩpɩɩ Adã do thueekɛ n 'laanɛnɩ yire.
46015046	Ga do thudaa dɔ cacadaa ga, sɩ tibil jaar gɩ, gɩrɛ dɔnɩ thudaa pɩɩrɔrɛ.
46015047	Caca tibil thɩɩra a the, thɩlãkobe Thãgba gba a mɩɩ, sɩ balanyɔ tibil ƴũ a the.
46015048	Mɔ̃ thɩlãkobidaar hanɩ, mɛ̃ thɩlãkobidara ha dakha, dɩ mɔ̃ ƴũdaar hanɩ, mɛ̃ ƴũdara ha dakha.
46015049	Dɩ mɔna sɩ kɔɔ donɩ thɩlãkobidaarɩ hoho, mɛ̃ sa do dakha ƴũdaarɩ hoho.
46015050	Gɩrɛ mɩ sonɩ wɔɔ omɩnaa dʋɔn: Tomɩ nʋʋn na tɔmɩn na puno na lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dʋɔa', dɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa na puno na 'lɛ dakha gɩrɛ na kʋɛanaa ga.
46015051	Hιnɛ thɩ̃ gbul gι dι ɩ̃ so, ga do sɛrɛ fɛʋ na daarɛ daanιkɛ dɔnι khirə', sι fɛʋ sa debire dapaara,
46015052	mɔ̃ tibil n canι yinə pɩpɩɩ tutuu ʋʋnna. Gɩdonɩ tutuu na ʋnɛ, dɩ khe na ɩɩr na tomɩrɩkɛ na dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa ga, sɩ sɛrɛ sa debire.
46015053	Gɩdonɩ dɔ tomɩ kʋɛnaakɛ n to gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa ga, dɩ tomɩ khinəneekɛ n to gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ dakhinənə'.
46015054	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tomɩ kʋɛnaakɛ na tonɩ gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa ga na pɩ, dɩ tomɩ khinəneekɛ na to gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ dakhinənə' na pɩ, le thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ kherenenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Kəəre gbaar khir a dɩɩ” na dã dɩphã.
46015055	“Khir ya, ka afɩ kəəra ha? Khir ya, ka afɩ kpalla ha?”
46015056	Khiri kpal dʋɔn sopugo, dɩ sopugoo fãga dʋɔn jɔfʋ.
46015057	Sɩ Thãgba hɩna fʋɔrɛ, ɔrkɛ n hana sɩnɩ kəəre, dɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira gɩ-n the.
46015058	Mɛ̃ gɩ ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, nɩ fɔ gɩ ma, na-n ha tutugo paara', na-n dɔ thɔma Kɔ̃tɩnna wire wire gɩ bɔr ga-n pɛr, gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ anɩ thɔna Kɔ̃tɩnna na do mɔlɔ kpɩɩraka'.
46016001	Ado warraakɛ nɩ pɛnɩ tɩɩ phuusɔra gɩ, mɔ̃kɛ mɩ kɔɔ pɛrnɩ gɩ hana Galasɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔɔ pa, nɛrɛ dakha nɩ cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃.
46016002	Nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl, caca wire fɛʋ wire makonyɔra, nɩ te gɩrɛ nɩ-n 'lɛnɩ a na thɩnɛ; ga-n too ɩ̃ pɔ dɩphã sɩ war n tea'.
46016003	Dɩ a mɩ pɔr tɩbɩlaakɛra na tini, wɛr ma ha sɛbɛ, wɩ jalana na anɩ khaardara Jerujalɛm.
46016004	Dɩ ado gɩ teenanɛ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n jala dakha, wɩ cʋrna mɩ sɩ jal.
46016005	Ma pɔr anɩ pa sɩ Masedʋan ma kɔɔ the ɓo, gɩdonɩ Masedʋan ma kana.
46016006	Agakpaana ma toore anɩ pa gbe, anaa ma toorerakɛ dɩ ie bɔɔ na kana, dɩ mɛ̃ na thɔɔ mɩ ka ma-n jalnɩ.
46016007	Gɩdonɩ nɛnɛ̃ ma ƴaal ɩ̃ yɩ nɩ sɩ ɩ̃ kpãsa', sɩ mɩ pɛrɛ haar ma toona nɛr gɩ ma gbe ado Kɔ̃tɩn tu.
46016008	Sɩ Efɛjɩ ma too na dana fɛtɩɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Pãtɩkotɩ,
46016009	gɩdonɩ lõfonɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ khɛr marɛ hoo, ɩ̃ puno ɩ̃ do le bɔ taa thɔma, sɩ lãlara jɔrɛ.
46016010	Ado Timothe pɔ, nɩ dɔ a toona nɩ sɩ maar na fʋʋa', gιdonι ɩ̃ kha a-n do Kɔ̃tιnι thɔ̃.
46016011	Na-n do tibil n 'lũə koe. Nι thɔgɔɔ na ha ιι a bir a ɩ̃ ɩ̃ pa, gιdonι mι-n pιɛrʋʋrɛ nakha omιna.
46016012	Sι ado Apolɔsιιkɛ dɔnι omine gι, mι kɔɔ bιɛlʋʋlɛ ka dι a na pɔ anι pa, nakha omιna, sι ɔɔ ƴaalla aa pɛr haar a pɔ nɛnã', sι ado a yι hʋɛ a na pɔr.
46016013	Na-n jʋrɛ, nι tɔɔ ha pɛrɛra kιbι, nι hana kũu bιnɛ, nι 'lɛ fãga na pιɛr.
46016014	Dɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ nι-n cʋʋnι na-n cʋʋ na naʋ.
46016015	Mι-n kpãkpãa narɛ gιrɛ wo omιna: Nι jιrɛ Sιtefanasι na ɔɔ cɔdara; caca tιbιla wɛɛkɛ 'lɛnι Akaι dιιra, a dona dakha wιrɛ faanι dιbara tιι phuusɔɔ bul thɔmana.
46016016	Nɛrɛ dakha a nι jι nι wuro jɔ wa tibil casɔraale, na wιrɛraakɛ n gbũgbuloneni kha thɔmana na wɛr.
46016017	Mι-n kãkarɛ Sιtefanasι, na Fɔrtunatusi, na Akaιkusii ιna, wɛr lona anι ba mɛ̃.
46016018	Gιdonι wι cʋʋrɛ dι ɩ̃ ha ie na anɩda dakha; nɩ gba wa tibil casɔɔle wɩ do nar tibil.
46016019	We gbɛbɩdaraakɛ hanɩ Ajɩ fʋɔr nɛr. Akɩlasɩ na Pirisika na we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ n gbɛbanɩ kha awɩ cɔ fʋɔr nɛr jɔɔ Thãgba bɩsã fʋɔrɛ.
46016020	Omɩna fɛʋ fʋɔr nɛr. Na-n fʋɔrɛ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl na ha lõ fʋɔrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnɩ daphuu.
46016021	Mɛr Pol khera fʋɔrɛɛkɛ na ɩ̃ nyɛ̃.
46016022	Ado tibil yɩ, ɩna-n na Kɔ̃tɩna', dɔ sʋɔn n 'lii. Maranata: Ɩna ya asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃.
46016023	Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn na-n jɛ nɩ bʋɔra.
46016024	Mɩ na nɛr fɛʋ dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the.
47001001	Mɛr Polɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni, na Timotheekɛ dɔnɩ omine, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ hanɩ Korɛ̃tɩ na tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ paar fɛʋ Akaɩra.
47001002	Thãgba asɩ Thɩ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn n hana nɩ ha ɩɩ a jɛ nɩ dakha bʋɔra.
47001003	Thãgba asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii Thɩ hɩna fʋɔrɛ, Thɩrɛ gɩ kɛ bʋɔ n fʋnɩ, a dor dakha Thãgbaakɛ ha faarɛ fɛʋ n thernɩ.
47001004	Ɔr n cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sa-n faa haar asɩ nɩra fɛʋ, dɩ mɛ̃ ha faarɛɛkɛra sɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n 'lɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa, sa punone ɔmɛ̃ a na cʋʋ wɩrɛ n yɛnɩ nɩ caar wo nɩ caar dɩɩdɩɩ, dɩ wa faa haar.
47001005	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ-n 'lɛnɩ Kirisitii gaar jɔɔ, mɛ̃ dakha sɩ-n 'lɛ ha faarɛ jɔɔ dɩ a-n the Kirisitirara.
47001006	Ado sɩ-n yɩrɛ nɩwɛ hananana, anɩ ha faa na anɩ taa 'lɛ dɔ kɩrʋ; dɩ ado sɩ 'lɛ ha faarɛ, anɩ ha faa dɔ kɩrʋ, kɛ na ba cʋɛ nιnι dɩ na fʋ haar bɔ gaar ca bɩɛllaakɛra sɩ-n yɩnɩ dakha ser.
47001007	Dɩ asɩ nũ pɛ nɛrɛra na ha baal paara', gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ bulni kha na sɛrɛ bɔ gaarɛ, mɛ̃ na bul kha na sɛrɛ ha faarɛ.
47001008	Omɩna, sa-n ƴaal na-n jɩ mɔ̃kɛ gɩrɛ hanaa ga: Nɩwɛ kɔɔ dã sɛr Ajɩra waa, dɩ sɩ kɔɔ gbɛ̃gbɛl dɩɩ thʋ̃ kãasɩ asɩ fãgara, sa thʋ̃ jɩrakɛ sa hananɛ yire bã.
47001009	Sɩ kɛrakɛ asɩ bɩnɔ ser yɩ khikhi togʋʋ sɩ too, dɩ mɛ̃ sa pɛ asɩbara haar mɔ̃kɛ sɩ donɩ thɩ̃a', sɩ sɩ pɩɛr Thãgba haar, ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛnɩ khe dɩ wɩ ɩɩr a the khirera.
47001010	Ɔr gɩɩkɛ kɔɔ taa sɩnɩ, dɩ ɔrra na taa sɩ khi puurəəkɛ; ɔrra sɩ hananɔ nũ pɛrɛ dɩ a na taa sɛr wo.
47001011	Nɛrɛ dakha n bulo si na Thãgba bɩɛlɛ, dɩ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛra sɩ-n 'lɛnɩ tibil jɔjʋɔɔ Thãgba bɩɛllala na dor nɔɔ, dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ na khɩɩ Thãgba asɩdara.
47001012	Gɩdonɩ asɩ məbida dʋɔn sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ asɩ kpɩɛrnɔ n ha sɩnɩ, dɩ sa-n ɩɩrna tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ thɩ̃thɩɩn na phur na fɩlɛɛkɛ hanɩ wasɩ, kɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara, sɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn jɔ; sɩ ga do tibil kpɛsɛrɛra gɩ tha', sɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩra gɩ-n the.
47001013	Sa khere nar dɩkha kpɩɩ, sɩ ga do gɩrɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ sɛbɛra na gɩrɛɛkɛ na jɩnɩ kɩrʋ gaaga. Nɩ kɔɔ jɩrɛ asɩda gbe, dɩ mɩ pɛrɛ haar na jɩrɛ tue bɔɔbɔɔ na dana khu paar,
47001014	dɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wirə sɛr na dɔ nar məbidaa mɔ̃kɛ na do sarnɩ məbidaa.
47001015	Ga tu jɩɩlera dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ ƴaalla gɩ do anɩ pa mɩ kɔɔ pɔ ɓo, dɩ mɛ̃ na 'lɛ balanyɔ kãkar,
47001016	sɩ ɩ̃ the anɩ pa ɩ̃ jal Masedʋan, sɩ ɩ̃ bir ɩ̃ the Masedʋan wo ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa, nɩ thɔɔ mɩ dɩphã ma-n jal Jude.
47001017	Dɩ mɔ̃ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ thalera, khʋma khʋma tibil ha maa bɛ? Agɩbo gɩ ho mɔ̃ tibili tibil do pa hanɩ ɩ̃ ƴaal n jal, gɩ ho “ɔɔ” na “ooho” har ɩ̃ pa ya?
47001018	Mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba donɩ sobɔdaar, mɛ̃ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ na kɔɔ do “ɔɔ” na “oohoa'.”
47001019	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa Bikuun Jeju Kirisitiikɛ mɛrɛ na Sɩlvɛ̃ na Timothe kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ ɔɔda anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, na kɔɔ do “ɔɔ” dɩ “ooho” ga, ɔrra wer “ɔɔ” haar gɩ dɩbara.
47001020	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa ʋlfɛsɔ fɛʋ “ɔɔ” gɩ do ɔrra. Dɩ gɛr gɩ, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ sɩ-n gbanɩ dɩ sa-n sona “amɛn” Thãgbaa i na-n dʋbɩrɔ.
47001021	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛ sɩnɩ nakha nɛrɛ dɩ sɩ tɩ Kirisitira, kɛ kɔɔ phire sini dakha, Thãgba gɩ.
47001022	A pɛ sarɛ dakha ɔɔ jẽ, a pɛ asɩ hara Thu Phuu dɩ do barã paar gɩrɛraakɛ sa 'lɛnɩ.
47001023	Mɔ̃ ga fʋnɩ sɩɩ do gɩ bul ner dɔ nɔɔ ma kɔɔ birni pɔ Korɛ̃tɩ dɩɩra ga, dɩ Thãgba to garɛ yire dɩ sobɔr mɩ so.
47001024	Sɩ ga nɩna fãga sɩ-n ƴaal sɩ cʋʋ nar ha pɛdaara ga, sɩ sɩ-n ƴaalɛ sɩ bul kha anɩ da hanana, gɩdonɩ nɩ tɩrɛ ha pɛrɛra.
47002001	Mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ kɔɔ te kpɩɛrɛ kɛ ɩ̃ bɩnɔ sa yɩ, ma bir na pɔ anɩ pa gbobirera ga.
47002002	Gɩdonɩ ado mɩ cʋʋ nι dι nι gbobi, amɛ na cʋɛ daʋ dι a fʋ mι saagado ʋrɛra mι cʋʋnɩ dɩ gbobi ga.
47002003	Mɩ kɔɔ khere narɛ gɩrɛɛkɛra mɩ kɔɔ kherenɩ, dɩ a ma pɔ anɩ pa, ma-n yɩ gbobire wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ na cʋɛnɩ wo dɩ daʋ na fʋ ma'. Dɩ mɩ hananɛ ga ha pɛɛkɛ, dɩ ɩ̃ daakɛ na fɔ mɩnɩ na dɔ nɛrɛ fɛʋʋda.
47002004	Gɩdonɩ gbobi kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, na ha helle, na yilẽbe jɔɔ mɩ kherena nar sɛbɛɛkɛ, ga do dɩ ma cʋʋ nɩ nɩ gboba', sɩ dɩ na jɩ dɩ naʋʋkɛ mι hana narnι gι kɔ̃tιnɛ.
47002005	Ado tibil do nɔɔ dι gbobire hale, ga do mɛr dιbara a cʋʋ dɩ ɩ̃ gboba', sɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ gɩ; sɩ anaa ga do fɛʋ ga, mɩ sor thakɛ gɩdonɩ ma-n ƴaal ɩ̃ kaya ɩ̃ dɛɛnɔa'.
47002006	Sorɩkɛ ɩkhasɔ bərəəm nɛrɛra kɔɔ pɛrnɩ kuunnaale daan.
47002007	Gɩ baar dɩ na ka na faa ɔɔ sopugo na haa dɩphã, sɩ na ƴɔlʋʋ haar, agado mɛ̃ ga, ha dɩ gbobire na thʋnɛ na jʋɔraa.
47002008	Mɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr dɩ na nɩnaa naʋ.
47002009	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dakha dɩ ɩ̃ khere nar, a be nɩ bɩnɛ ma-n hɩɩn, ado na nɩrɛ nũu thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
47002010	Sɩ ntɛɛ sopugookɛ nɩ-n faanɩ, mɩ-n faarɛ mer. Sɩ ado mɛrra gɩ, gɩrɛ mɩ-n faanɩ, ado ger mɩ kɔɔ faarɛ dɩkhaa sopugo, nɛr dɔ nɔɔ Kirisitii ƴɛra.
47002011	Dɩ mɛ̃ Satã na yɩ sar hʋɛa', gɩdonɩ jɩɩr na 'lee sɩ ɔɔ fɩɩlla ga.
47002012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ danɩ Tʋrʋasɩ ɩ̃ mɩɩ Kirisitii tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ khɛr mɛr loo wer,
47002013	sɩ ɩ̃ ha na kɔɔ jɩɩl cɔcɔa', gɩdonɩ ma kɔɔ yɩ Tɩtɩ ɩ̃ oma', dɩ mɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ hʋɛ sa gba jal Masedʋan.
47002014	Thãgba hɩna fʋɔrɛ, ɔrkɛ n cʋɛ sɩnɩ wire koo dɩ sa-n kəə, dɩɩ do Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ gba sɩ dɩ cʋʋna dι jιιrιkɛ tιbιla na jιnι Kirisiti na-n pι paar fɛʋ mɔ̃kɛ latιkolo n hʋnι.
47002015	Gιdonι ado Thãgbara gι, sι hʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnanι daʋ, dι Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ, wιrɛ 'lɛnι taarɛɛ thɩ̃thιιn na wιrɛ n buurenii thɩ̃thιιn.
47002016	Wɛra wer, khi hʋnɛ gι-n do war dι a-n jalna wι khirrə, sι ado wɛra wer, yi hʋnɛ gι-n do war dι a-n jalna wι yirera. Dι ʋmɔ̃ dana thɩɛnaale?
47002017	Gɩdonɩ sa ho tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ n mɩanɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ dɩ wa-n pɛ awɩ kũkunoə', sɩ ha phuu ser n mɩɩna, mɔ̃ sɩ donɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔna Thãgbaa ƴɛra, a ha Jeju Kirisitira.
47003001	A thɩɛna gaa, sɩ bire ma sa-n nɩna asɩbara dɩ tɩɩ teenaa sɩ doaa bɛ? Dɩ agɩbo ʋkhasɔɔ kha sa ƴaal tetee sɛbɛ sɩ nɩna nɩ, agɩbo sɩ ba ƴaal nar?
47003002	Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛra ka do asɩ sɛbɛ, a khere asɩ hara, dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ jɩ gɩ dɩ wa-n hɩɩn.
47003003	Sɛbɛɛkɛ Kirisiti kherenɩ nɩ do gbelẽ gbelẽ, kɛ sɩ doronɩ thɔ̃ dona. Ga do sɛbɛ khere nƴʋɔn wɩ kherena ga, sɩ Thãgba yidaarɩ Thu gɩ kherena, ga do boka thelnaana gɩ khera', sɩ tibil haarra gɩ khere.
47003004	Gɛr dɔ tu jɩɩrɩkɛ sɩ hananɩ Thãgbara dɩɩ the Kirisitira.
47003005	Ga do sɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ hɩna punone a na ba kpɩɛr dɩkha gɩ ho asɩ pa gɩ tha', sɩ asɩ puno Thãgbara gɩ-n the.
47003006	Ɔr hana sɩ punone dɩ sɩ do thɔ̃ dona nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ phaara, ga do jɔfʋraakɛ kherenenɩ gɩ bã, gɩdonɩ jɔfʋʋkɛ kheranɩ n kʋrɛ, sɩ Thu Phuu n 'laanɛ yire.
47003007	Gɩdonɩ ado jɔfʋ 'laarɛɛkɛ kherenenɩ bokaarra kɔɔ ιnanɛ khir sιι dorakɛ gι kɔɔ ιιrnanɛ carbararɛ dιι do Thãgbaa i dʋbιra gι the, dι Ɩjιrayɛl bιsana na-n ba puno na jιι hιιn Mʋιjιι ƴa', gιdonι ɔɔ ƴɛ carbaraalera dɔ kιrʋ, sιι dorakɛ dakananɛ gι,
47003008	na jι dιι do thɔmaakɛ dɔnι Thu Phuuda n carbararɛ a ka gelaa?
47003009	Ado so heen thɔma hananɛ carbara caale, ga do fιl sar thɔma na-n carbararɛ ka gι jɔ gele fĩiəə?
47003010	Mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ hanι thaa, gιrɛra n kɔɔ carbaranɛnι na do thɩ̃ɛ bã, gιdonι gιrɛ jɔ gιnι fĩi na carbararɛ ιnɛ a thi gar.
47003011	Dι ado gιrɛ dɔnɩ dakananɛ kɔɔ hananɛ carbararɛ, dɩ mɔ̃ gɩrɛ n tɔɔnɩ khorrɩ carbara na ha?
47003012	Dɩ mɔ̃ sɩ hananɩ ga nũ pɛ caakɛ, sɩ-n mɩɩrɛ na 'lar casɩ.
47003013	Sa-n cʋʋ Mʋɩjɩɩ kha ga, kɛ kɔɔ gbaannɩ kɩ̃kɩɩn a thi ɔɔ ƴɛra, gɩ do nɔɔ Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsana na-n ba hɩɩn kirkirkir gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dakananɛ gɩ dana khu paaraa ga.
47003014	Awɩ kpɩɛr dibi warɛ, gɩdonɩ a dana nĩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n sonɩ ʋlfɛ tɩ̃ sɛbɛ, kẽkẽ ca gelela bor hale 'lo ga tə', gɩdonɩ Kirisiti dɩbara na te gɩ dɩ a ther.
47003015	Sɩ a dana nĩkɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ wɩ-n sonɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ sɛbɛ, kɩ̃kɩɩn n hale awɩ hara dɩɩ kɛɛ.
47003016	“Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil n kɛrnɩ da-n kpa Kɔ̃tɩnna, kɩ̃kɩɩn n tire.”
47003017	Dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn, Thu Phuu gɩ; dɩ ka Kɔ̃tɩnɩ Thu n hanɩ, le wa dʋʋr n ha.
47003018	Dɩ gɛr gɩ sɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na hananɩ dɩkha dɩɩ kɛɛ sɩ ƴιɛra bã, Kɔ̃tɩnɩ carbara n caranɛ sɩ ƴɛ bire mɛ̃ hɩɩn khaa, dɩ sɩ debi na hʋʋ a na pɛr, dɩɩ do Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ Thu Phuu pa gɩ-n the.
47004001	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ hananɩ thɔ̃ ca ƴɩrɛ, mɔ̃kɛ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ sɩ 'lɛnɩ hanɩ, nyɛ̃ɛ na-n khiir sa'.
47004002	Sɩ-n bor yicur thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n cʋɛnɩ wolonena, dɩ sa-n ɩɩrna fɩɩla', dɩ sa-n golõ dakha Thãgbaa thɩmɩa', sɩ sobɔ sorra casι sι-n nιnana Thãgbaa ƴɛra, tibil caar fɛʋʋ kpιɛrra, dι tibil teena sι do.
47004003	Sι adorakɛ asι tutugo bɔ thιmιι bo ker, wιrɛraakɛ n buureni gι ker,
47004004	kɛ dɔnι ha pɛ 'leedara, kɛ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ thãgba yaarnι awι kpιɛr, wa-n puno a yι tutugo bʋɔɔ dahιra', kɛ dɔnι tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ n nɛnanι Kirisitii i dʋbι, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ n kureni kha na Thãgba.
47004005	Ga do asιbara sι gba sa-n mιι mɔ̃ sι hana', Jeju Kirisitii Kɔ̃tɩ̃ do sι-n mιι, na mɔ̃ sι donι anι thɔ̃ dodaarsɔ dιι do Jeju dɔ nɔɔ.
47004006	Gιdonι Thãgbaakɛ sɔnι ayι, dahιrɛ n caranɛ dabirəə thɩ̃thιιn, ɔr cʋɛ dahιrɛ dιι carã asι hara, gι cʋʋ tibil a jι Thãgbaa i dʋbιιkɛ Kirisiti n nιnanι.
47004007	Sι hananɛ ga tιι ko thɩ̃ιkɛ daaraakɛ dɔnι ja daa, dι mɛ̃ fãgaakɛ na hanι mιɛrɛra ga, ga dor Thãgba hιna, ga do asι pa gι tha'.
47004008	Nιwɛ fɛʋra sa-n yι fɛfɛɛ paara', sι sa ha tiirrə na tə'. Kpιɛrɛ nyanyãa sɛr ka, sι sa-n faa nũ pɛra'.
47004009	Wι-n kpoo sarɛ sι Thãgba na bo sa'. Wι-n thʋna sɛr thιι, sι sa wιɛla'.
47004010	Wire fɛʋ paar fɛʋ, asι tomι n khi Jejuu khi, dι mɛ̃ dakha Jejuu yi na yιr asι tomιra.
47004011	Gιdonι sɛrkɛ hananɩ yire, bɔɔ fɛʋra wɩ-n to sɩ khirrə dɩɩ do Jejuuda dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ Jejuu yi na yɩr asɩ tomɩraakɛra dɔnɩ dakhinəne.
47004012	Mɛ̃ gɩ, khir n dʋɔn thɔma sɛrɛra, sɩ yire n puno a na-n do thɔma nɛrɛra.
47004013	Ha pɛ ca bɩɛlla sɩ hana mɔ̃kɛ gɩrɛ kheranɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra sonɩ ayɩ: “Haar mɩ kɔɔ pɛr, gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ mɩɩ”, sɛrɛ dakha haar sɩ pɛr gɛr gɩ dɩ sa-n mɩɩ.
47004014	Gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn khirera, a na ɩɩr sɛr dakha na Jejura, a kpa sɩ sɩ jɩɩl kha na nɛrɛ ɔɔ ƴɛra.
47004015	Gɩdonɩ gelela fɛʋ nɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ a-n ha, dɩ mɛ̃ bɔ jɩɩr na-n dɛbɩrɔ gɩ cʋʋ Thãgba khɩɩrɛ jɔɔ n hale tibil jɔjʋɔra, Thãgbaa i na-n dʋbɩrɔ.
47004016	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ nyɛ̃ɛ na-n khiir sa', gɩdonɩ adorakɛ asɩ tomɩɩkɛ na kʋɛrɛ, sɩ asɩ tibil ʋrɛ hanɩ bɩnɔ, kɛ na dɔnɩ dayɩnana', n debire dɩ do daphaa da-n pɛr wire fɛʋ.
47004017	Gɩdonɩ asɩ nɩ jaba jabaakɛ sɩ-n yɩnɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ gbe, har dɩ a-n ɩna sar i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ khorrdaa.
47004018	Gɩdonɩ ga do gɩrɛ tibil n yɩnɩ na yire ser n hɩɩna', sɩ gɩrɛ tibil na punoni na yɩ na yirə' sɩ-n hɩɩn. Gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ tibil n yɩnɩ na yire dakananɛ gɩ, sɩ gɩrɛ tibil na punoni na yɩ na yirə' khorrdaa gɩ do.
47005001	Gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do ado asɩ tomɩ kɛ thɩɩra, kɛ dɔnɩ waa wɩɛl, sɩ hananɛ le Thãgbaa dʋɔ cʋɔrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa nyɛ̃ thɔ̃, khorr too paar gɩ, ga do tibil nyɛ̃ɛ ma'.
47005002	Sɩ dakha sɩ-n thʋnɛ sa-n 'wɩɩ waʋʋkɛra ka, dɩ sa-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ sɩ mʋa asɩ Thãgbaa dɩ cɔra,
47005003	gɩdonɩ a sɩ 'li mʋʋrɛ pι, wa yι sι gι do sι 'leere tomιra'.
47005004	Gιdonι sɛrkɛ hanι wa ʋrɛraakɛ, sι-n 'wιιrɛ sι gbɛ̃gbɛlnι, dι sι-n ƴaalɛ ga do dι sa for thιιkɛɛ tomι na fa ga, sι dι sa to ƴũ tomɩr, dɩ mɛ̃ ga dor yire gbaan gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dakhinəne a dɩɩ.
47005005	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ cʋɛ sɩnɩ a pɛ gelelala, Thãgba gɩ, kɛ kɔɔ hana sɩnɩ Thu Phuu dɩ do barã paar gɩrɛraakɛ sa 'lɛnɩ.
47005006	Gɛr gɩ wire fɛʋ sɩ-n hananɛ tu jɩɩr, dɩ sɩ jɩrɛ mɔ̃ sɩ-n cɔnɩ tomɩrraakɛ, sɩ toore a hʋnɔna Kɔ̃tɩn.
47005007	Gɩdonɩ ha pɛrɛra sɩ-n ɩɩr, ga do yi yɩrra ga.
47005008	Gɛr gɩ tu jɩɩrɩkɛra sɩ hananɩ, ƴaal kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dʋɔn, sɩ faa tomɩrɩkɛ sɩ hananɩ sa jala a tɔɔna Kɔ̃tɩn.
47005009	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dakha dɩ sa-n do bʋɔ, sɩ sɩ daaraa haar, ado sɩ-n toore kɛ tomɩrraakɛ, a sɩ-n fagʋʋrɛ.
47005010	Gɩdonɩ dɔ sɛrɛ fɛʋ n jal sɩ jɩɩl Kirisitii kɩɩl too pa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, wɩ nɩrɔ mɔ̃ sɩ hanɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl na 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ dɩ a ha mɔ̃ ntɛɛ bɔ cʋʋ, na ntɛɛ puu cʋʋ hanɩ, a hanɩkɛ tomɩrra.
47005011	Dɩ sɩ jɩnɩ gɩrɛ n dɔnɩ sɩ ma Kɔ̃tɩn, sɩ-n ƴaalɛ sa-n yɩrana tɩbɩla, Thãgba jɩ sɛr casɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ hanɩ, dɩ mɩ pɛrɛ haar anɩ kpɩɛrnɔra nɩ jɩ sɛr dakha mɔ̃kɛ sɩ hanɩ.
47005012	Sa bir ma sa-n nɩna asɩbara nɛrɛra dɩ tɩɩ teena sɩ doa', sɩ hʋɛ sɩ ha nɩ dɩ na məbi asɩdara, dɩ na puno na birse wɩrɛɛkɛ n məbəni gɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ yi yιdaa, sɩ ga-n do hadaa ga.
47005013	Gɩdonɩ ado sɩ də̃bəəl Thãgbaada dɔ nɔɔ, sι ado sι jιrɛ fιlɛ nɛr dɔ nɔɔ.
47005014	Gιdonι Kirisitii naʋ n tɔ sɩ, gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩɛ jɩ dɩ ado bɩɛl kɔɔ khire tɩbɩlala fɛʋ, ga dor dι tɩbɩla fɛʋ khiire.
47005015	Dɩ ɔr kɔɔ khe tɩbɩlala fɛʋ, dɩ mɛ̃ wɩrɛɛkɛ n hananɩ yire, wa hana yire wa-n nana dɩbara ga, sɩ gɩ dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ khe warnɩ sa ɩɩr a the khireraada.
47005016	Mɛ̃ gɩ, a fʋna nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã, sa-n hɩιn tibil mɔ̃kɛ tɩbɩla thɩɩra n hɩɩnna'. Dɩ adorakɛ thalee hɩɩn sɩ kɔɔ jɩna Kirisiti, sɩ ga do mɛ̃ sɩ jɩɩ gɩrɛ bã.
47005017	Ado tibil ha Kirisitira tibil phaa a-n do, thɩ̃ tɩna phor ka, hιnɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ n debire dɩɩ do daphaa.
47005018	Dɩ gele fɛʋ Thãgbara gɩ the, kɛ cʋɛ sɩnɩ dɩ sɩ bir kũu kha na ɔr dɩɩ the Kirisitira, dɩ ha sɩ bir kũu kha thɔma.
47005019	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba kɔɔ haan Kirisitira a cʋʋ tɩbɩla dɩ wɩ bir kũu kha na ɔr Thãgba, aa therna tɩbɩlaa dɩ pa ga, wo a pɛ sarɛ sa-n mɩa bir kũu kha thɩmɩɩr.
47005020	Sɛr dʋɔn Kirisitii dedeesɔɔkɛ Kirisitira thɔnɩ, dɩɩ ho sɛr Thãgba n gba da-n kpãkpaana dɩ yɩ: Sɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr Kirisitii irə, nɩ birə kuune kha na Thãgba.
47005021	Kirisitiikɛ na kɔɔ jɛnɩ sopugoə', ɔr a cʋʋ dɩ debi do sopugo dɩɩ do sɛr dɔ nɔɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ sɩ debi do fɩl sarʋ Thãgbara, dɩ Kirisitira gɩ the.
47006001	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ-n donɩ kha thɔma na Thãgba, sɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr dɩ na-n do Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ na do nar thɩ̃aa ga.
47006002	Gɩdonɩ a sor ayɩ: “Bɔɔkɛ gɩ teenɩ kha mɩ kɔɔ pɛ fɛr nũu, tataa wire mɩ kɔɔ bul fer.” Hɩnɛ, nɛnɛ̃ dʋɔn bɔɔkɛ gɩ teenɩ kha. Hɩnɛ, nɛnɛ̃ dʋɔn tataa wire.
47006003	Sa-n pɛ nɛ baradaa tibillə thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ bɩɛllalaka', gɩ ho thɔmaakɛ na hananɛ kpɛ paara'.
47006004	Sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, asɩ fɩl n nɩna dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃dara sɩ do, ha fʋrɛraakɛ sɩ-n hananɩ jɔɔ nɩwɛra, na gɩrɛraakɛ telene sɩnɩ, na mɔ̃ sa-n yɩnɩ fɛfɛɛ paara',
47006005	na bɩɩrɛra, na khaɩ pɛrra, na dɩ nyanyaanɛna, na thɔ̃ khe dʋʋrra, na yi cɔnanɛna, na kɔmɛr cɔnanɛna,
47006006	dɩɩ the dakha fɩl phuurə, na jɩɩrra, na ha fʋ yɩrrɛra, na ha bulo fɩlɛla, na Thu Phuurə, na naʋ bʋɔra,
47006007	na sobɔ thɩmɩɩrra, na Thãgbaa fãgara, na fɩl sar ko ke thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ sɩ-n pɩɛrnanɩ a dona gɩrɛ sɩ-n phinəni tomɩr;
47006008	na dakha i dʋbɩrɛra, na beesirera, kuerera na i bɔ werra; fɩfɩla wɩ-n we sɩ, sɩrakɛ sobɔ so tɩbɩla ha sɩ.
47006009	Wa jɩ sa', sɩrakɛ tɩɩ jɩnanɛ bɔɔbɔɔ ha sɩ; wɩ yɩ sa jɩ paar na pɔa', sɩ sɛrkɛ na yire; wɩ yɩ sɩ-n yɩrɛ naarɛ, sɩ ga do sa khirə';
47006010	wɩ yɩ gbobire wɔɔ sarɛ, sɩ wire fɛʋ daʋ n fʋ sɛr; wɩ yɩ bɔdara ha sɩ, sɩ sɛr n lɛ tɩbɩla jɔɔ; wɩ yɩ sa hana thɩ̃a', sɩ sɛr hɩna thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
47006011	Korɛ̃tɩdara wei, sa mʋ̃ nar dɩkha ga, sɩ faarɛ haar yala a ha nɩ.
47006012	Asɩ naʋ na 'lũə', sɩ anɩda 'luno.
47006013	Nι faa haar yala a ha sι mɔ̃ sι faanι asιda a ha nι, mι mιιna nɛr mɔ̃ nι donι ɩ̃ bιsãsɔ.
47006014	Na-n tu kpele bιɛl tʋʋr na wιrɛ dɔnι ha pɛ 'leedara ga. Gιdonι anyee bɔ ca fιl sarʋ na fιl gõgolõ na-n bɔ kha? Anye dahιrɛ na dabirə ha kha?
47006015	Anyee 'li ca Kirisiti na 'linə kha Belιal? Anyera ʋrɛ pιɛrnι haar na ʋrɛ na pιɛrnι haara' na bul kha?
47006016	Anyee gbɛbι ca Thãgbaa cɔ na gbɛbι na thιla? Gιdonι sɛr dʋɔn cʋɔr Thãgba yidaarra, mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ sonι ayι: “Ma toore awι bιnɔ, ma-n kpaarɛ awι thɩ̃thιιn. Ma dor awι Thãgba, dι wa dor ɩ̃ too.”
47006017	Gɛr gι, “Nι thɛ awι thɩ̃thιιn, nι lea hana kpιι, Kɔ̃tιn sɔ. Na-n tha gιrɛraakɛ bisenenə', dι mɛrɛ ma tee ner,
47006018	dι ma do narɛ Thιrɛ, dι nɛrɛ na do marɛ bikona na bikhɛna, mɛr Kɔ̃tιn fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar sɔ.”
47007001	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mι-n nanι, mɔ̃kɛ sι hananι ʋlfɛ ca gιrɛ, sι phʋɔlɛ khorr gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n biseneni tomιr na thue, a na bãbanɛ na asι kpιι lee Thãgba maarra.
47007002	Nι tea sι na haar. Sa dι tibillə ga, sa kʋɛ tibilə', sa phʋʋn tibil woa'.
47007003	Ga do sor mι-n heen nι mι mιιnι thakaa koe. Gιdonι mι kɔɔ 'lire sor ayι: Sι fʋ nɛr na haar, a sι har kha kɛ na yire, a sι-n khire kha.
47007004	Mι hana narɛ ha pɛrɛ jɔɔ ka. Mι hananɛ məbidaa ka nɛrɛra, ha ƴɔllɛ ha marɛ vʋ̃ʋ, daʋ thʋnɛ ka mar asι bɔ gaar fɛʋʋ thɩ̃thιιn.
47007005	Gιdonι a fʋna bɔɔkɛ sι kɔɔ danι Masedʋan sa kɔɔ yι hιιrɛ fιιʋraka', sι sι kɔɔ gaarɛ bʋɔ thɩ̃ɛ dιιdιιra. Kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ jιɛra, maar bιnɔ.
47007006	Sι Thãgbaakɛ n cʋɛnι wιrɛ kpιɛrɛ nyanyaanι dι wa-n faa haar, ɔr kɔɔ cʋɛ dι Tιtɩɩ ɩ̃ do nɔɔ dɩ sɩ faa haar.
47007007	Sɩrakɛ ga do ɔɔ ɩ̃ιle dɔ nɔɔ dɩbara ga, sɩ gɩdonɩ Tɩtɩɩ thɛthɛ 'lɛr ha faarɛ anɩdara, a mɩɛ sɛr mɔ̃ nɩ-n ƴaal mɩnɩ ka, a mɩɛna anɩ gbobi, na mɔ̃ anɩ gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ mɛrɛra hanɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ daʋ fʋ mɩ dɩphã waa a ka.
47007008	Sɩrakɛ ɩ̃ sɛbɛ cʋʋ nɩnɩ dɩ nɩ gbobi sɩ ma so a ma ja', gɩdonɩ mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩ sɛbɛɛle cʋʋ nɛr dɩ nɩ gbobi, sɩ bɔɔ gbe gɩ.
47007009	Dɩ adorakɛ mɩ kɔɔ sor a ma jɩ, sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ gɩ da marɛ, ga do gɩdonɩ nɩ gbobire ga, sɩ gɩdonɩ anɩ gbobi thɔɔ nɛr pɛ ha debirera. Gιdonι mɔ̃ Thãgba ƴaalnɩ nɩ kɔɔ gbobi, dɩ mɛ̃ ga do sɛr pɛ nar ga soole fɩɩʋraka'.
47007010	Gɩdonɩ gbobire mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni n ɩnanɛ ha debire, kɛ n thɔɔnɩ tibil dɩ pɛ taarɛra, dɩ ha debi ca ole na hana tibil n soro a ma ja'; sɩ gbobireekɛ dɔnɩ thɩdaa khir gɩ-n ɩna.
47007011	Gbobi ca ʋrɛ hanɩ mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni, nɩ hɩnɛ gɩrɛ gɩ cʋʋ narnɩ ɓoɓo dɩ nɩ pər waa gel, na mɔ̃ nɩ gbuuni thɩmɩɩrraale yʋʋ, na mɔ̃ gɩ hel nɩnɩ haar, na mɔ̃ maar fʋ nɩnɩ, na mɔ̃ anɩ ƴaal kɔ̃tɩ̃ hanɩ, na mɔ̃ anɩ gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ hanɩ, na mɔ̃ anɩ thɩ̃ naar hanɩ. Dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋraakɛ nɩ nɩna dɩ na hana dɩɩ thɩmɩɩrraala'.
47007012	Ado mɩ kɔɔ khere narɛ ga do ʋrɛ cʋɛnɩ puureele, agɩbo dɩ ʋrɛ wɩ cʋʋrɔnɩ puureele mɩ khereroa', sɩ gɩ do nɔɔ nɩ jɩ anɩbara Thãgbaa ƴɛra mɔ̃ anɩ pər sɛrɛra hanɩ.
47007013	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ sɩ kɔɔ faa haar; sɩ asɩ ha faara kãkar n pɛrɛ jɔɔ, dɩɩ the daʋraakɛ kɔɔ fɔnɩ Tɩtɩ, gɩdonɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ daʋ fʋʋ.
47007014	Sɩ ado anɩda dɩkha kɔɔ dor nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ məbiro Tɩtɩɩ ƴɛra, ƴicuru na kɔɔ fʋ ma', gɩdonɩ mɔ̃kɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ donɩ sobɔr, mɛ̃ asι məbi Tɩtɩɩ ƴɛra ha, dɩ sobɔrra wɩ yɩ gɩ dɩɩ do.
47007015	Naʋʋkɛ a hananɩ nɛrɛra n pɛrɛ jɔɔ, mɔ̃ a-n jɩnanɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋʋ nũ nι, na teereekɛ nι kɔɔ teguuni na maar na jẽu.
47007016	Gɩ da marɛ mɔ̃ mɩ hana narnɩ tu jɩɩr thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
47008001	Omɩna, sɩ cʋʋ nɛr nɩ jɛna Thãgbaa bɔ jɩɩkɛ yɩranɩ Masedʋan we gbɛbɩdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn.
47008002	Bɔ gaarɛɛ mɩɛ kɔ̃tɩnaakɛ wɩ kɔɔ hanɩ, awɩ daakɛ jʋɔnɔnɩ na awɩ bɔdaar do phuphuphul, pɛ warɛ ha bulo thɩ̃ 'laarɛ dɩɩ kãasɩ.
47008003	Mɩ punone so wɩ kɔɔ 'laarɛ na haar kpẽgelẽ mɔ̃ awɩ puno hanɩ, wɩ kɔɔ 'laarɛrakɛ dɩɩ ka jɔ mɔ̃ awɩ puno hanɩ.
47008004	Wɩ kɔɔ bɩɛl sɛr na haar fɛʋ aa, hʋɛ n hanale ɩnɩ-n puno iner ɩnɩ-n har tɩɩ phuusɔɔ bul thɔnana.
47008005	Wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ jɔ gɩrɛ sɩ kanɩ kɔɔ kpɩɛr, sɩ awɩbara wɩ kɔɔ faa a ha Kɔ̃tɩn ɓo, dɩ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba tuni wɩ kɔɔ faa awɩbara dakha a ha sɩ.
47008006	Gɛr gɩ sɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlɛ Tɩtɩ dɩ na pɩɩr anɩ pa ga ha bulo thɔ̃ caale mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ ɩɩrna gɩnɩ.
47008007	Mɔ̃kɛ gɩdonɩ thɩɛna fɛʋ nɛr n jɔ, ha pɛrɛra, thɩmɩɩrra, jɩɩrra, na pərre dɩɩdɩɩra fɛʋ, na anɩ naʋraakɛ thɛnɩ asɩ pa, ɔmɛ̃ nɩ dɔ wɩrɛ na jɔnɩ ga ha bulo thɔ̃ caraale.
47008008	Mɩ sonɩ thakɛ ga do jɔfʋ mɩ-n pɛ nara', sɩ ɩkhasɔɔ pər mɩ gba a bena nɩ bɩnɛ dɩ ma-n hɩɩn ado anɩ naʋra sobɔr gɩ do.
47008009	Gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii bɔ jɩ, mɔ̃ a kɔɔ donɩ lẽledaar sa tu a do bɔdaar anɩ sora, dɩ ɔɔ bɔdaar dora na cʋɛ nɩ dɩ na le.
47008010	Ɩ̃ kpɩɛrnɔ mɩ ha nɩ dɩbara dɔrɔɔm gɩdonɩ gɩ teere kha, gɩdonɩ a fʋna ƴakhɛrɔ nɛr kɔɔ kʋlɛ ƴɩɛ, ga do thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra dɩbara ga, sɩ ƴaalɛla dakha.
47008011	Gɛr gɩ nɩ pɩrɛ gɩrɛra nɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnι, dι mɔ̃kɛ nι kɔɔ gʋʋrnι na haar fɛʋ gι hana, nι cʋɛ gι gι pι mɔ̃kɛ anι puno hanι.
47008012	Ado tibil 'laa thɩ̃ɛ na haar fɛʋ mɔ̃ ɔɔ puno hanι, gɛr n da Thãgba haar, sι ga do gιrɛ ntɛ na hananaa wι soaa dɛ.
47008013	Ga do dι ga pɛ nar bʋɔ sι gι ba ιkhasɔra ga, sι gι cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ gɩ mãkha kha.
47008014	Nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ anɩ thɩ̃ jɔ hana n bulle awɩ thɩ̃ ɓɔr, dɩ mɛ̃ dakha awɩ thɩ̃ jɔ hana na bul anɩ thɩ̃ ɓɔr, dɩ mɛ̃ mãkhar na hale,
47008015	mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ khɩanɩ jɔɔ na hana thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ kara', dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ khɩanɩ gbe thɩ̃ɛ na ɓɔrʋa'.”
47008016	Thãgba hɩna fʋɔrɛ, gɩrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ pɛrnɩ Tɩtɩɩ hara dɩ hana nar ga pər ca bɩɛlɩkɛra.
47008017	Gɩdonɩ a ture asɩ bɩɛl, sɩ ɔɔ ƴaalla gɩ kɔɔ therakɛ mɔ̃ a-n pərni jɔɔ ka dɩ a na pɔ le na yɩ nɩ.
47008018	Sɩ-n thɔnaanɛ kha omineekɛ hananɩ i bʋɔ we gbɛbɩdara fɛʋʋ thɩ̃thɩɩn tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra.
47008019	Wo, we gbɛbɩdara kɔɔ phiiruure a dɔ asɩ kpakpaar ga ha bulo thɔ̃ cʋʋraakɛra sι-n cʋʋnι, ga-n dʋba Kɔ̃tιnι thɛthɛɛ i, ga-n nιnana dakha mɔ̃ asι ƴaal bɔ hanι.
47008020	Gιdonι sa ƴaal tibil n pɛ sar sor mũsũ jɔraakɛ wι dʋ sιnι nyɔ̃kɔa'.
47008021	Gιdonι sι-n ƴaalɛ gιrɛ bʋɔnɔnι, ga do Kɔ̃tιnι ƴɛra dιbara ga, sι dakha tιbιlaa ƴɛra.
47008022	Sι-n thɔna wɛr dakha asι omi ʋrɛ sι kɔɔ jιιnι jʋʋr ɔɔ pər thɩ̃ɛ dιιdιιra a hιιn, kɛ n nɛnanι nɛnɛ̃ dakha mɔ̃ ɔɔ pərra jɔɔ hanι, dιι the ha pɛrɛraakɛ a hananι nɛrɛra.
47008023	Sι ado Tιtι gι, ɔr dʋɔn ɩ̃ bubul na ʋrɛ sι-n donanι kha thɔma anι pa. Sι ado asι omisɔ wɛ, we gbɛbιdaraa thɔ̃thɔna ha wι na Kirisitii i dʋbιdara.
47008024	Dι gɛr gι nι nɛna wι we gbɛbιdaraa ƴɛra mɔ̃ anι naʋ hanι, na hʋɛɛkɛ sι kɔɔ hananι anιdara dι sa-n məbi.
47009001	Ado gιrɛraakɛ dɔnι tιι phuusɔɔ bul thɔ̃ gι, ma laar 'lo na khere nar sɛba'.
47009002	Gιdonι mι jιrɛ anι ƴaal bɔ, dɩ gɛr mɩ-n məbiro anιdara Masedʋandaraa thɩ̃thιιn a so war ayι: Akaιdara kɔɔ gbɛbιrɛ pι kɛkɛkɛ ƴakhɛrɔ. Dι anι gbɛ̃gbɛrɛna kɔɔ jaa tibil jɔjʋɔ.
47009003	Mι-n thʋɔn omιna dι mɛ̃ anιdaakɛ mι-n məbironi gelelala na do mɔlɔa', dι dakha wι yι nι nι gbɛbιrι nι pι mɔna mι kɔɔ sonι.
47009004	Ado mɛ̃ ga, sι dι sι pɔ kha na Masedʋandara dι na gbɛbι a pa', ga dor mɔ̃ sι yιnι sι jιrɛ anι ti, na dor asι yicur na anιda.
47009005	Mι kɔɔ kpιɛrɛ gι bɔrɛ gɛr gι dι ɩ̃ kɔɔ bιɛl omιna wι kʋʋl nι ƴιɛ wι pɔ anι pa, wι kɔɔ gbɛbι ha bulo khaardaakɛ nι kɔɔ 'lini sor na 'laarɛ; mι-n ƴaalɛ gι dɔ ha bulo khaardaa ga-n ho bɩ̃ puudaa ga.
47009006	Nι jɛ ʋrɛ direni fιιʋ, fιιʋra a na kha, sι ʋrɛ direni jɔɔ, jɔɔra a na kha.
47009007	Tιbιla fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl na-n 'laanɛ mɔ̃ ntɛɛ bɩ̃ kpιɛr hanι, wa-n 'laa na gbobira', ga-n ho tɔ pɛr gι woa'; gιdonι Thãgba n nar ʋrɛɛkɛ n 'laanɛnι na kãkar.
47009008	Thãgba hananɛ punone a na bɔna nι na bɔna caar fɛʋ dιιdιι, dι mɛ̃ na-n hana wire fɛʋ gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na-n dana nιnι, na hana gɛr dι a jɔr na ka, na-n cʋʋna thɔ̃ bʋɔ fɛʋ,
47009009	mɔ̃kɛ gι kherenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Ha bulole a-n 'laana khaardaa jɔɔ bɔdarara, ɔɔ fιl sar khorr gι too.”
47009010	Ʋrɛ n 'laanɛnι be bi jaldaarra na dιkɔ a khɔ, ɔr na 'laanɛ be na ha nι dι a dɛbιrɔ, dι ɔr na cʋɛ dι ha bulo be na se nar ga-n pɛr.
47009011	Dι mɔ̃ nι hananι thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ na punone na-n 'laa thɩ̃ɛ na ha bulole, dɩ anι khaardasɔɔkɛra sι-n 'laanι ga 'laarɛ Thãgba khιιrɛ.
47009012	Gιdonι bul thɩ̃ɛɛkɛra n 'laanɛnι, ga do tιι phuusɔ gι-n bul thɩ̃ ɓɔrɛra dιbara ga, sι dakha ga tɔr Thãgba khιιrɛ jɔɔ ga-n pɛr.
47009013	Ga bul thɔ̃ɔkɛ n nɛna mɔ̃ nι hanι, dι wa-n khιι Thãgba anι nũ nιra mɔ̃kɛ nι tuni Kirisitii tutugo bɔ thιmιι, na ha bulo thɩ̃ 'laarɛraakɛra n nɛnanɩ anɩ kũu bɩnɔ do na wɛr, na tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
47009014	Dɩ wɩ-n bɩɛlɛ Thãgba dɩ wa-n pɛ nar gɩdonɩ nɩ lõ wer haar, dɩɩ the bɔ jɩɩrraakɛ thʋnanɩ kar, kɛ Thãgba jɩ nɩnɩ.
47009015	Thãgba hɩna khɩɩrɛ ɔɔ khaardaraakɛ na hanɩ mɩɛrɛra ga.
47010001	Mɛr Pol, mɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr na hɛlɛlɛ fιlɛ na bɩ̃ bʋɔraakɛ dɔnι Kirisitiida, mɛrkɛ n hanι hɛlɛlɛ a mι ha anι thɩ̃thιιn, sι a mι hʋnɔ ma-n 'la nι kpãkpalã ga.
47010002	Mι-n ƴɛɛ nɛr dι na-n do ɔbɔɔkɛ ma hanι anι pa, ma ιιrna narɛ 'larιkɛ mι hananι a kpιɛr ma ιιrnanɛ ιkhasɔraakɛ n kpιɛrɛnι aa, mɔ̃kɛ tibili tibil do pa hanι sι-n ιιra'.
47010003	Tibil sι do wer, sι ga do mɔ̃kɛ tibili tibil do pa hanι sι-n kɛ̃kɛrã'.
47010004	Gιdonι ko ke thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ sι-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnanι ga do tibildaa ga, sι Thãgba dɔ nɔɔ dιι hana fãga ka, a na puno gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ datutugonaa ga a na wɩɛl. Sɩ-n bũburonanɛ mɔlɔ kpɩɛrɛsɔ,
47010005	na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n ɩrɛnɩ na gũ tir dɩ a-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna Thãgba jɩɩr, sɩ-n fʋrɛ kpɩɛrɛ fɛʋ dɩ sɩ khɩmɩnɔ ga-n nɛ Kirisiti nũu.
47010006	Sɩ gbɛbɩrɛ pɩ dɩ sa heen nũ nʋra sor ɔbɔɔkɛ anɩ nũ nɩ danɩ.
47010007	Nɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ hanɩ. A tibil n kpɩɛrɛ Kirisitiida ɩnɩ do, dɔ a bir a kpɩɛr ɔɔ bɩnɔ a hɩɩn, mɔ̃ a donɩ Kirisitiida, sɛrɛ dakha Kirisitiida sɩ do ser.
47010008	Gɩdonɩ adorakɛ ma məbire dɩ a kãasɩ gbe hʋ hananɛnaakɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ, gɩ cʋʋ nɩ nɩ khɔ̃ na-n pɛr ga do gɩ kʋɛ na', yicuru na fʋ ma'.
47010009	Ga do mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ ho mɩ-n phərə ner na ɩ̃ sɛba'.
47010010	Wɩ-n sor dɩ wɩ yɩ, ɔɔ sɛbɛ khɩɩrɛ ka, ga-n gɔ kpãkpalã ga, sɩ a fɩ yɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛ, sʋmʋmʋ̃ a ha dɩ ɔɔ nɔ thɩmɩɩ mɔlɔ thɩmɩa yɛ.
47010011	Dɔ ntɛɛle n mɩanɩ thale n jɩ: Mɔ̃ asɩ thɩmɩɩ n hanɩ sɛbɛra ado sa hala', mɛ̃ dakha asɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ n ha ado sɩ hale.
47010012	Sa 'la na gba asɩbara na mɩɛna tibil ɩkhasɔɔkɛ n kpãganɛnɩ dɩbara ga, agɩbo sɩ yɩ sɩ jɛ ʋrɛ jɔna', mɔ̃ wɩ-n mɩɛnɩ dɩbara na awɩ mɩɛda awɩ ha wɩ jɩ ʋrɛ jɔnɩ, fɩlɛ ɓɔra wɩ.
47010013	Sɩ sɛrɛ, asɩ məbi na kãasɩ gɩrɛraakɛ sɩ kɔɔ cʋʋna', sι ka Thãgba yιnι sι dɔ asι thɔ̃ kho, le sι khu, dι anι pa gι khu.
47010014	Sa-n kãasι asι pɛla', gι ho sa kɔɔ pɔ a dã anι pa gaaga, gιdonι sɛr dɔ wιrɛ kɔɔ dana nιnι waa gel na Kirisitii tutugo bʋɔ.
47010015	Asι məbi na kãasι gιrɛraakɛ sι cʋʋna', dι sa məbi haanι thɔna ga, sι sɩ hananɛ nũ pɛrɛ anɩ ha pɛ n khɔna pɩɛr, sɩ yɩ hʋɛ asɩ thɔ̃ pɛl n tɔ gɩ pɛr,
47010016	dɩ sa mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔ anɩ billo, sɩ sa too sa-n məbi thɔmanaakɛ ʋkha kɔɔ 'lini cʋʋra', gɩ ha mɔna gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ:
47010017	“Dɔ ʋrɛ n məbəni, a na-n məbi gɩrɛraakɛ Kɔ̃tɩn cʋʋnɩ.”
47010018	Gɩdonɩ ga do ʋrɛ n kpãganɛnɩ dɩbara ɔr wɩ-n we tibilə', sɩ ʋrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn n kpãganɩ gɩ.
47011001	Ga da marɛ ado na punone na fʋ haar ɩ̃ mɩɩ də̃bəəle fɩɩʋ, sɩ nɩ-n fʋrɛrakɛ haar.
47011002	Gɩdonɩ gbugiikɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara fʋ mɛr anɩ sora, gɩdonɩ mɩ kɔɔ gba nɛr a ha kũu bɩɛl dɩ Kirisiti gɩ, dɩ nɩ dʋʋraa khɛ biir phuukɛ na jɛnɩ kuuna'.
47011003	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ sii kɔɔ fɩɩlnɩ Ɛvɩ na ɔɔ fɩɩlla, maar n fʋ mɛr dɩ anɩ kpɩɛr na kʋɛrɛ, gɩ kɛr sɩ gɩ faa sobɔr na phur Kirisitira.
47011004	Gɩdonɩ a tibil pɔ nar na mɩɩ nar Jeju kpɩɩ na ʋrɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ narnɩ, dɩ agɩbo nɩ 'lɛr Thue dɩ ha kpɩɩ na ʋrɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ, agɩbo tutugo bɔ kpɩɩ gɩ na gɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ teenɩ, nɩ-n fʋrɛ haar bɔɔbɔɔ.
47011005	Mɩ pɛrɛ haar ma 'lũ thɩ̃ bɩɛllalakɛ a jɔ wa thɔ̃thɔnaale bʋɔnɔnɩ ka ga.
47011006	Dɩ ado mɩ hor tibil ba thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛra, sɩ jɩɩr wer na ɓɔr ma', dɩ sɩ kɔɔ nɩna gɛr anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn tɩbɩlala fɛʋ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
47011007	Sopugo mɩ ba cʋʋ gɩrɛraakɛ mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔ khaar yaa? Mɛr wuro mɛ̃ sɩ ner n ka nɩ ɩɩr.
47011008	Ɩkhaa we gbɛbɩdarara mɩ kɔɔ 'lɛ bulle, wɛrra mɩ-n 'lɛ loka nɔɔ dɩ ma-n dona nar thɔma.
47011009	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ anɩ pa dɩ bʋɔ kɔɔ fʋ mɩ, ma kɔɔ do heendaa tibillə ga; gɩdonɩ omɩnaakɛ thɛnɩ Masedʋan n kɔɔ hana mɩ gɩrɛ n ɓɔra mɩnɩ. Dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra mɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ dɩbara dɩ ma do nar heendaa ga, dɩ ma fʋrɛ dɩbarararakɛ 'lo.
47011010	Sobɔrraakɛ n thɛnɩ Kirisitiraakɛ ha marnɩ, mɩ sor ayɩ: Thɩ̃ɛ na hale na tɔ̃ mɩ məbire ga thɩnaakɛ Akaɩ dɩɩra ga.
47011011	Mɔ̃ dɔ nɔɔ? Gɩdonɩ a thɩɛna gaa ma na naa ya? Thãgba jɩ gɛr.
47011012	Gɩrɛra mɩ-n cʋʋnɩ ma cʋʋrɛrakɛ ma-n jalna, dι mɛ̃ ga khaan hʋɛ wιrɛraakɛ n ƴaalɛnι hʋɛ wι yɛ sι mãkhanɛ kha gιrɛraakɛ wι-n məbironi.
47011013	Tιbιlaale sõso thɔ̃thɔna wɛ, dι fιfιιl thɔ̃ dona wɛ, dι wι debi ho Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔ̃sɔ.
47011014	Sι gele ga do nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ ga, gιdonι Satãa thɛthɛ n debire dι ho thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu hιrɛ.
47011015	Dι ga do nɔ kpaarɛ gι ado ɔɔ thɔ̃ dodaarsɔɔle debi a ho fιl sar thɔ̃ dona ga. Awι khu pa na har mɔ̃ awι thɔ̃ hanι.
47011016	Mι bire 'loro wo, tibil na-n hιιn mι ɩ̃ ho də̃bələ', dι a gι harakɛ mɛ̃, sι nι tea mι ɩ̃ dole də̃bəllə, dι mɛ̃ ma məbi dakha gbe.
47011017	Gιrɛ mι sonɩ gɩrɛ, ga do mɔ̃ Kɔ̃tɩn n ƴaalnɩ mɩ soa', sɩ gɩ hor mɔ̃kɛ də̃bəəle n ɩɩrnanɩ tibil dɩ mɩɩ thɩ̃ɛ, dɩ gɩrɛra mɩ-n məbironi tu jɩɩr harrɛ.
47011018	Gɩdonɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ hale n məbəni sɩɩ do awɩ məbira məbire gɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ tibili tibil do pada, mɛrɛ dakha ma-n məbire.
47011019	Gɩdonɩ nɩ-n fʋrɛ haar də̃bələla ka nɛrkɛ jɛnɩ fɩlɛ.
47011020	Ado tibil na pɔtɔrɔ nɩ, ado tibil na kho nɩ, ado tibil na tagɩrɩ nɩ, ado tibil na so nar kuune, ado tibil be nɩ ƴɩɛ, nɩ-n fʋ garɛ haar.
47011021	Yicuru fʋ mɛr dɩ ma so nayɩ: Sɩ kɔɔ nɩna nɛr mɔ̃kɛ asɩda na khɩɩrna'. Sɩ gɩrɛ tibil n kpãgarɔnɩ dɩbara, mɩ punone cʋʋ mɛ̃ mer, də̃bəəlela mι mɩɩ.
47011022	Ebirəsɔ ha wɩ ya? Mɛrɛ dakha Ebirəra ha mɩ mer. Ɩjɩrayɛldara ha wɩ ya? Mɛrɛ dakha. Abɩrahamɩ məl ha wɩ ya? Mɛrɛ dakha.
47011023	Kirisitii thɔ̃dara ha wɩ ya? Mɩ do ger dɩɩ jɔ mɛ̃, sɩ də̃bəəlela mɩ mɩɩ wo. Thɔ̃ khe dʋʋrra mɩ jɔ wɛr, khaɩ pɛrra mɩ jɔ wɛr, bɩɩrɛra mɩ jɔ wɛr fĩi, bɔɔ jɔɔjɔɔ mɩ-n thɔɔ khir.
47011024	Balamɔɩ Juifisɔ kɔɔ bɩɩr mɩ be nʋɔ kpalanyɔ phe bire.
47011025	Balãther wɩ kɔɔ ciil mi na khasa, babɩɛl wɩ kɔɔ dʋʋr mι na bokana, balãther gborõo kɔɔ mʋʋna mι, dι wi bιɛl na dιtɩ̃ bιɛl nyʋɔn kɔɔ gba mι dι ɩ̃ cʋʋ.
47011026	Ɩ̃ kpaarιkɛ mι-n kpaarnι gι jɔrɛ ka, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr mιιrra, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr yu hɔ̃hɔlaa pa, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr ɩ̃ caa pa, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr ca kpalaa pa, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr dιιra, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr bəənnə, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr lanyʋɔnna, nιwɛ nɔ mɛr wιrɛ n cʋɛnι wι yɛ omιna hanιι thɩ̃thιιn.
47011027	Mι jιrɛ gιrɛ n dɔnι thɔ̃ dʋʋr, na vɔɔrɛ, na yi cɔnanɛ bɔɔ jɔɔjɔɔ, na kɔmɛr na yɔlkhaa fʋʋr, na kɔmɛr cɔnanɛ bɔɔ jɔɔjɔɔ, na ie fʋʋr na kẽkẽ 'leere.
47011028	Thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔ hale na mιana', sι gιrɛɛkɛ heene mιnι a jɔrakɛ fɛʋ dʋɔn dɛrιkɛ mι-n hananι wire fɛʋ we gbɛbιdarara fɛʋ.
47011029	Ʋmɔ̃ na yɔɔnɛ sιι do ma yɔɔ mera? Ʋmɔ̃ na baranɛ na ji sιι do haar na hel ma?
47011030	Ado gι dor ɩ̃ məbə, ɩ̃ yɔɔda ma məbiro.
47011031	Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι Jeju Kɔ̃tιnι Thι, kɛ hιnanι fʋɔrɛ khorr, jιrɛ dι ma-n kur sõsora'.
47011032	Aretasι fãgadaarι gobanɛr kɔɔ pɛrɛ wa-n bɛra Damasι dιι a fɔ mι,
47011033	sι wι kɔɔ gbũ mer kpʋʋnɔ a tona fɛnɛtιrι dι ɩ̃ gbũ sortoto, dιι do mι taarɛ ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
47012001	Gι teenanɛ ɩ̃ məbi sιrakɛ ga-n hana khora', sι ma mιɛ nɛr thɩ̃ yιr na thɩ̃ nιrɔrɛɛkɛ Kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ cʋʋ mιnι dι ɩ̃ yι.
47012002	Mι jιrɛ tibil bιɛlιkɛ hanι Kirisitira, kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ vəni a jʋʋnna a dana balãther thãgbara ƴũ, yɛna yʋɔr yenã gι gιrɛ, ado tomιr a kɔɔ hana ya, ado tomιr gaa ya, ma ja', Thãgba jιɛn.
47012003	Dι tibilile ado tomιr a kɔɔ hana ya, ado tomιr gaa ya, ma ja', Thãgba jιɛn.
47012004	Mι jɩrɛ dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ gbaarɛ a lona hɩɩr paar Thãgbaa kal ƴɔɔ, dɩ a kɔɔ nɩrɛ thɩmɩaakɛ tibil na marnɩ na mɩa', kɛ tibil na hananɩ dakha hʋɛ a na mɩɛa'.
47012005	Ma məbire tibil caarra thale, sɩ ado mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛra wer, ma məbi saagado ɩ̃ yɔɔda gaaga.
47012006	Sɩ ado mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ məbi, ga do də̃bəl ma doa', gɩdonɩ sobɔr ma so, sɩ ma-n cʋa', dɩ mɛ̃ tibil na hana mar kpɩɛrɛ gɩ kãasɩ gɩrɛraakɛ wɩ-n yɩnɩ mɛrɛra, agɩbo gɩrɛraakɛ wɩ-n nɩnɩ mɛrɛra ga.
47012007	Mɔ̃ na dɔnɩ nɔɔ sɩ thɩ̃ nɩrɔ caale na hanɩ mɩɛrɛra ga na cʋʋ mɩ dɩ ma ti gunə', gɛr gɩ dɩ uu ga mar tomɩrra, kɛ dɔnɩ Satãa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar a na-n ʋ̃ʋ mar gɩ do nɔɔ ma ti gunə'.
47012008	Gelelala mɩ kɔɔ bɩɛl Kɔ̃tɩn balãther a cʋɛ gɩ gɩ hʋnɔ mar.
47012009	Sɩ a so marɛ ayɩ, bʋɔraakɛ ɩnɩ-n jɩ mɩnɩ gɩ daan, gɩdonɩ yɔɔrɛra ɩnɩ-n jɩɩ nɩna ɩnɩ fãga. Dɩ gɛr gɩ ma-n ka jɩɛ məbi na daʋ ɩ̃ yɔɔra, gɩdonɩ liir Kirisitii fãga n ha mar.
47012010	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ma-n kãka yɔɔrɛra, na nɩɩrɛra, na nɩwɛra, na kpoorera, na bɔ gaarɛra Kirisitii sora; gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ-n yɔɔnɩ, liir mɩ-n ka 'lɛ fãga.
47012011	Də̃bəl mɩ debi do, sɩ nɛr kɔɔ tɔ mɩ pɛr dɩ ɩ̃ ha mɛ̃. Gɩdonɩ anɩ pa gɩ kɔɔ teenana gɩ thɛ nɩ yɩ ɩ̃ tɩɩ teena do. Gɩdonɩ ma 'lũ fɩɩʋrakɛ a jɔ wa thɔ̃thɔnaale bʋɔnɔnɩ ka ga, sɩrakɛ ma do thɩ̃a'.
47012012	Gɩrɛ n nɛnanɩ ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar do, gɩ yɩrrɛ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn na ha fʋrɛɛkɛ jʋɔnɔnɩ ka, na jẽ thɩ̃ɛsɔ, na ma kʋ thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ, na nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ.
47012013	Anye kɔɔ ɓɔra nɩ sɩ dɩ wɩ̃ we gbɛbɩdara hana gɩ a jɔ nɩ, saagado gekɛ ma kɔɔ do narnɩ heendaa gaaga. Dɩ nɩ faa ɩ̃ dɩɩdɩɩ hɩɩnna ha mɩ.
47012014	Hɩnɛ, mɩ gbɛbɩrɛ gɩrɛ pɩ ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa balãther pʋɔr, sɩ ga do heendaa ma do nara', gɩdonɩ ga do anɩ thɩ̃ mɩ-n ƴaala', sɩ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ gɩ. Gɩdonɩ ga do bɩsana teana wa-n thɩnɛ thɩ̃ɛ a hana thɩrɛ na nɩra', sɩ thɩrɛ na nɩrɛ teana wa-n thɩnɛ thɩ̃ɛ a hana awɩ bɩsãsɔ.
47012015	Sɩ ado mɛr gɩ, mɩ ture na haar ɩ̃ 'laa gɩrɛ mɩ hananɩ, ɩ̃ 'laana dakha dɩbara koo gɩ do anɩda thuerə dɔ nɔɔ. Dɩ mɔna mɩ-n na nɩnɩ mɛna dɩɩ thʋ̃ kar, gɩ dor nɔɔ dɩ anɩ naʋ na-n wurəə bɛ?
47012016	Sɩ anaa na sor wo nayɩ, ma kɔɔ do nar heendaa wera', sɩ mɔ̃ mɩ donɩ tɩɩ fɩɩl tibil, gɛr mɩ kɔɔ fɩɩl nar sa 'li ni.
47012017	Tɩbɩlaakɛ mɩ kɔɔ thɔnɩ anɩ pa, mɩ ba phiro sɩ ma-n kho nɩ yaa?
47012018	Tɩtɩ mɩ kɔɔ bɩɛl a jala anɩ pa, dɩ mɩ kɔɔ thɔnaanɛ dakha omi bɩɛl. Dɩ Tɩtɩ ba khɔ nɩ yaa? Ga do kpɩɛr bɩɛlla sɩ ha kha na ɔraa? Ga do nɛ ka bɩɛlla sɩ-n 'loro kha gaa?
47012019	Nɩ kɔɔ mãa kpɩɛrɛ kɛkɛkɛ dɩ sor sɩ-n hɛl dɩbara nɛrɛra. Kirisitira sɩ ha dɩ sa-n mɩɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra. Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ wei, gelela fɛʋ anɩ khɔ̃ pɛ sɩ-n ƴaal.
47012020	Gɩdonɩ maar fʋ mɛr dɩ anaa a ma dã le, ma yɩ nɛr dɩ na ha mɔ̃ ma-n ƴaalna', nɩ yɩ mɩ dakha ɩ̃ ha mɔ̃ na-n ƴaalna'. Maar fʋ mɛr dɩ anaa kɩla, na gbugi, na nĩkhii, na dɩbara na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ, na tibil kuere, na wɩ yɩ mɩɩrɛ, na i kaar, na nyanyaanɛ na har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
47012021	Maar fʋ mɛr dɩ a ma dã le, ɩ̃ Thãgba na cʋʋ mɛr dɩ yicuru na bir na fʋ mɩ anɩ sora, ĩ tha ɩ̃ thʋnɔ sɩ ma-n bɩ wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ maanɩ cʋʋrɛ sopugo, sɩ ɩkhasɔ wɛrra na kɔɔ debi haar thɩ̃ bise cʋʋrɛraalera, na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra, na dakhaba cʋʋrɛra ga.
47013001	Balãther ha gɩrɛ mɩ-n pɔnɩ anɩ pa. “Sɔ ɓibi na gʋʋrɛ mɔ̃kɛ sobɔ so jɩdara yenyɔ agɩbo yẽther yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ ha”, thale gɩ khere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra.
47013002	Balanyɔ pʋɔrɩkɛ mɩ kɔɔ pɔnɩ anɩ pa, mɩ kɔɔ 'lire so gar, na ninəkɛ ma hanɩ gɩrɛ anɩ pa ga, mɩ maanɛ gɩrɛ dɩ ma-n so wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ maanɩ cʋʋrɛ sopugo, dɩ mɩ-n sor dakha tɩbɩla fɛʋra ayɩ: Ado mɩ bir na pɔ anɩ pa, na-n yɩ ma pɩrrɛ fɩɩʋrakaa koe.
47013003	Gɩdonɩ nɩ-n ƴaalɛ nɩ jɩ gɩrɛ n nɛnanɩ dɩ Kirisiti n mɩana mɩ, ɔrkɛ na yɔɔnɛ narna', sɩ a-n nɩnanɛ ɔɔ fãga anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
47013004	Sobɔr gɩ wer, wɩ kɔɔ kpaarɛ thɩrʋra ɔɔ yɔɔra, sι a hananɛ yire gιrɛ dιι the Thãgbaa fãgara. Dι sɛrɛ dakha ɔɔ khara sι yɔɔ, sι sa hananɛ kha yire na ɔr gι the Thãgbaa fãgara, dι mɛ̃ sa puno sa-n do nar thɔma.
47013005	Nι mιɛnɛ anιbara na hιnɛ ado nι har ha pɛrɛra, nι jʋrɛ dιbara na hιnɛ. Na jι gι anιbara dι Jeju Kirisiti har anι bιnɔaa? Agado nɛr jʋrɛ dιbara a yιɛ dιι do nι 'leera'.
47013006	Sι mι pɛrɛ haar nι jιɛ jι dι asι dιbara jʋʋr wer na do sar 'leera'.
47013007	Sι sι-n bιɛlɛ Thãgba dι na-n cʋʋ dιkha gι puuro fιιʋraka', sι ga do sι-n ƴaalɛ sι yιra gι ho wι yɛ sɛr 'la', sι asι bιɛl dʋɔn na-n cʋɛ gιrɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnι adorakɛ asι 'li bire ho 'leere.
47013008	Gιdonι sa hana sobɔ pιɛr fãga ga, sι sobɔrι dabɔ ha sι hana.
47013009	Sι-n kãkarɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ sι hanι yɔɔrɛra, sι ne wer khιιr. Dι gιrɛ sι-n bιɛlnι Thãgbara dʋɔn mɔ̃ na jιιnι bɔr.
47013010	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dι ɩ̃ khere nar gιrɛ sι sa ha kha ga, dι mɛ̃ ɔbɔɔkɛ sa hanι kha ga teena ɩ̃ cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ na fãga ga. Kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ ha mɛr hʋɛ ɩ̃ cʋɛ nι nι khɔ̃ na-n pɛr, ga do nι kʋɛa ga.
47013011	Sι gιrɛ sɛnι dʋɔn wɔɔ omιnaa, na-n hana daʋ, na-n yιrana bɔrɛ ka, na-n ƴɔla kha haar, na-n hana kpιɛr bιɛl, na-n tɔɔ kha na ha ιι, dι Thãgbaakɛ naʋ na ha ιι n thernι, na-n har kha na nɛrɛ.
47013012	Na-n fʋɔrɛ kha bιɛlbιɛl na ha lõ fʋɔrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnι daphuu. Tιι phuusɔ fɛʋ fʋɔr nɛr.
47013013	Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιn na-n jɛ nι bʋɔra, Thãgba n cʋɛ nι na-n jι ɔɔ naʋ, Thu Phuu n cʋʋ nɩ kũu kha na ɔr ga-n pɛr; thale mɩ-n ƴaal gɩ hana nar fɛʋ.
48001001	Mɛr Pol thɔ̃thɔn, sι ga do tιbιla kɔɔ pɛ mara', dι tibili pa gι the woa', sι Jeju Kirisitii pa gι the, na Thãgba Thιrɛɛ pa kɛ kɔɔ ιrɛɛnι khirera;
48001002	mɛrɛ na omιna fɛʋʋkɛ sι hananι kha thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ Galasι we gbɛbιdarara.
48001003	Thãgba asι Thι na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιn, n hana nι ha ιι a jɛ nι dakha bʋɔra.
48001004	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ 'laanɛnι dιbara asι sopugosɔra a puno a ti si nɛnɛ̃ bɔ puurəəkɛ mɔ̃ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι asι Thι tuni;
48001005	ɔɔ i n dʋbarɔ na jala waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
48001006	Nʋɔ kpaa mɛr mɔ̃kɛ nι faanι dapaara ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ wɛ nιnι dιι the Kirisitii bɔ jιra, sa bir kɛr na-n hιιn tutugo bɔ kpιι,
48001007	sιι dorakɛ tutugo bɔ kpιι na hala'; sι tιbιla haanle dι wa-n bũburõ ni kpιɛrɛ, dι wι-n ƴaalɛ ιnι-n deba Kirisitii tutugo bʋɔ.
48001008	Dι ado sɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ gιrakɛ, dι ado Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu gιιkɛ thɛnι ƴũ n mιa nar tutugo bʋɔ dιι ha kpιι na gιrɛɛkɛ sι kɔɔ mιιnι, dɔ sʋɔn n 'lii.
48001009	Sι kɔɔ mãa sor, sι dι mι birrakɛ ma-n 'loro gιrɛ wo, ado tibil na mιι nι tutugo bʋɔ dιι ha kpιι na gιrɛɛkɛ nι kɔɔ 'lɛnι, dɔ sʋɔn n 'lii.
48001010	Dι nɛnɛ̃ tιbιla mι-n ƴaal wa-n khιa mι yaa, Thãgba mι-n ƴaal a na-n khιa mι? Agιbo tibil mι-n ƴaal ɩ̃ da haar kã? A ma ƴaal 'lo ma-n da tιbιla haar ma do Kirisitii dea'.
48001011	Mι so narɛ gιrɛ omιna, dι tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ mι kɔɔ mιιnι, ga do tibildaa ga;
48001012	gιdonι ga do tibili pa mɩ kɔɔ 'lɛ ga, dɩ tibil kɔɔ dιrɛ mι woa', sι Jeju Kirisitii nιrɔra mι kɔɔ 'lɛ gι.
48001013	Gιdonι nι kɔɔ nιrɛ mɔ̃kɛ ɩ̃ fιl kɔɔ hanι mamara ɔbɔɔkɛ mι-n kɔɔ fʋɔrnι Juifi Thãgba fʋɔrɛ, dι ma-n kpoo gbõgolonena Thãgbaa we gbɛbιdarara dιι ho ma hərə wer,
48001014	na mɔ̃kɛ mι-n kɔɔ fʋɔrnι Juifi Thãgba fʋɔrɛ a jɔ tibil jɔjʋɔɔkɛ dɔnι ɩ̃ 'walãkhasɔɔkɛ sι donanι kha ca bιɛl, na mɔ̃ mι kɔɔ hananι dakha gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛ ɩ̃ mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ sora.
48001015	Sι Thãgbaakɛ kɔɔ thιnɛ mιnι kpιι ɩ̃ nιι kɔ̃lora a we mι dakha ɔɔ bɔ jιra, dι ɔbɔɔkɛra gι kɔɔ daaraanι haar,
48001016	a gbaar ɔɔ Bikuun a nιna mι ɩ̃ gbaanɛɛ na mιa ca kpala, gɛr gιrakɛ dapaara ma kɔɔ therna tibilə',
48001017	dι ma kɔɔ jal dakha Jerujalɛm a yι wιrɛ kɔɔ kʋlɛ mιnι ƴιɛ a do thɔ̃thɔna ga, sι Arabι mι kɔɔ jal, agιpι dι ɩ̃ kɛr bir Damasι wo.
48001018	A yɛna yẽther ka, gɛr mι kɔɔ jaal Jerujalɛm sι jι kha na Pιɛr, dι mι kɔɔ cɔr le ɔɔ pa wire yʋɔr yemɔι;
48001019	sι tιι kpιιsɔɔkɛ dɔnι thɔ̃thɔna ma yι bιɛllakɛ saagado Jakι Kɔ̃tιnι õkuun gaaga.
48001020	Gιrɛ mι khere narnι gιrɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra gι, ma sõsoaa koe.
48001021	Sι a gι pιrɔ, mι gbaar jal Siri dιιra na Silisi dιιra.
48001022	Sι Jude we gbɛbιdaraakɛ hanι Kirisitira na kɔɔ to mar yirə';
48001023	dιbarara wι nιɛ ayι: Ʋrɛɛkɛ n kɔɔ kpoone sarnι mamara hale nɛnɛ̃ da-n mιι ha pɛrɛɛkɛra a-n kɔɔ yιrnanι kʋɛrɛ;
48001024	dι wι-n kɔɔ khιιrɛ Thãgba ɩ̃ sora.
48002001	A yɛna yʋɔr yenã ka, mι bire jal Jerujalɛm nakha Barnabasι, dι mι kɔɔ kpar dakha Tιtι dι sι ha kha.
48002002	Sι thɩ̃ nιrɔrɛɛkɛ thɛnι Thãgbara mι kɔɔ yι, gɛr gι dι ɩ̃ kɔɔ jal. Dι mι kɔɔ gbaar tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ mι-n mιιnι ca kpala a mιɛ wι dι wι hιιn; sι wιrɛ dɔnι yʋʋ wɛr mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ hɛllɩ, agado mɛ̃ gaa, ga hor thɔmaakɛ mɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnι, na gιrɛ mι hanι cʋʋrɔ gιrɛ, na dor mɔlɔ thɔma.
48002003	Dι Tιtιιkɛ sι kɔɔ hananι kha Gιrɛkι gι, sι tibil na kɔɔ fɛrɛɛrakɛ a kuro khʋ̃a'.
48002004	Dι ka kpιɛrɛɛle the, wιrɛ n yɛnι omιna hanιι pa gι, kɛ kɔɔ wolonenι a lõ asι thɩ̃thιιn dι wa-n gιιl asι waʋ do Jeju Kirisitira, dι awι ƴaal dʋɔn sι birə dɔ dea.
48002005	Sι sa kɔɔ tha thʋnɔ a 'larrakɛ sa tu awιda fιιʋa', gι do nɔɔ tutugo bʋɔ na-n jalna ɔɔ sobɔra ƴɛrr anι thɩ̃thιιn.
48002006	Wιrɛ wι-n hιιnnι dι wɛr dɔ yʋʋ, a wι kɔɔ har mɔ̃ wɩ hanɩ yo, ga do gele mɩ-n hɩɩna', Thãgba na-n hɩɩnnɩ tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa', wɩrɛ wɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ dɩ wɛr dɔ yʋʋ, wa kɔɔ hana dakpɩɩ na dɛbɩ ɩ̃ dɩɩrra ga.
48002007	Sɩ mɔ̃ wɩ kanɩ yɩɛ dɩɩ do mɛr Thãgba pɛr ma-n mɩa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ wɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa', mɔ̃ Thãgba pɛrnɩ Pɩɛr a na-n mɩa Juifisɔra,
48002008	gɩdonɩ ʋrɛra hananɩ Pɩɛr punone dɩ do thɔ̃thɔn Juifisɔra, ɔrra dakha hana mι punone dι ɩ̃ do thɔ̃thɔn ca kpalala,
48002009	dɩ mɔ̃ wɩ yɩnɩ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ Thãgba jɩ mɩnɩ bʋɔra hanɩ, Jakɩ na Sefasɩɩkɛ n dɔnɩ Pɩɛr, na Jã, kɛ wɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ dɩ wɛr dɔ thɩkara, wɩ kɔɔ fʋɔrɛ mɛrɛ na Barnabasɩ bɩɛl do fʋɔrʋʋ, mɔ̃ sι donι kha kũu bιnɔ, sι puno sa-n jal ca kpalaa pa, sι wɛr wa-n jal Juifisɔɔ pa.
48002010	Gιrɛ wι so sarnι dιbara dʋɔn sa-n jɛna nι bɔdara, dι mι kɔɔ ture na haar fɛʋ dι ma-n cʋʋ.
48002011	Sι ɔbɔɔkɛ Pιɛr kɔɔ pɔnι Ãtιyɔsι, mι kɔɔ bor ɔɔda kpei ma mʋʋnaa ga, gιdonι a heene sor dɩbara.
48002012	Gιdonι ɔbɔɔkɛ ιkhaa tibilsɔɔkɛ thɛnι Jakιι pa na kɔɔ pɔnι pa', ca kpala a-n kɔɔ khona dιkɔ, sι bɔɔkɛ wι danι, a-n mə̃mə̃ləne dι tɔ dι khokhιa, gιdonι maar n fʋɔnɛɛ wιrɛraakɛ n bɔnι dι wa-n ιι khʋ̃ kurrera.
48002013	Dι wɩ̃ Juifisnɔ phɛl a wolõ dι wa-n cʋʋ, dι awι bιnɛ yenyɔ fιlla ba hal Barnabasι dι lʋʋn.
48002014	Dι mɔ̃ mι yιɛnι dιι do wa-n ιιr dιι telẽ mɔ̃kɛ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnι sobɔr hana', mι kɔɔ sor Pιɛrra tιbιla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra ayι: Ado fɛrkɛ dɔnι Juifi hana ca kpalaa fιl, sι fa hana Juifi fιla', mɔ̃gιdo dι fa-n fɛrɛ ca kpala wɩ hanana Juifi fιlɛ?
48002015	Ado se wer, Juifi dʋʋr wι kɔna sι, sa do sopugodara mɔ̃kɛ ca kpala hana'.
48002016	Sιrakɛ sι jιrɛ dι ga do jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra tibil na 'lɛr so hɛlla', sι ha pɛrɛ Jeju Kirisitira gι; sɛrɛ dakha sι kɔɔ pɛr Jeju Kirisiti haar sor n hɛla sar, gι the ha pɛrɛraakɛ sι hananι Kirisitira, ga-n do jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra gι tha', gιdonι tibil bιɛllakɛ na 'lɛ so hɛllɛ jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra ga.
48002017	Sι mɔ̃ sι-n ƴaalnι sor n hɛla sar Kirisitira, sopugodarara sι do ser, dι Kirisiti ba cʋɛ sι dι sι do sopugodara kã? Kpei.
48002018	Gιdonι ado mι bir na mι gιrɛɛkɛ mι kɔɔ wιɛlnι, ɩ̃ sopugodaar do mι-n nιna.
48002019	Me wer, jɔfʋʋ sora mι khirore, gι do nɔɔ ɩ̃ hana yire Thãgbara.
48002020	Wι kɔɔ kpa mɛr kʋkʋ thιrʋra nakha Kirisiti, dι ga do mɛr gιιkɛ hananι yire gιrɛ bã, sι Kirisitiikɛ hanι ɩ̃ bιnɔ dɔ ɩ̃ yi; sι yireekɛ mι hananι gιrɛ, ha pɛrɛra mι hana gι Thãgbaa Bikuunnaakɛ n naan mιnι a ba faana dιbara ɩ̃ sora.
48002021	Ma bo bɔ jιιrιkɛ thɛnι Thãgbara ga, gιdonι ado jɔfʋra so hɛllɛ n the ga dor khaar Kirisiti kɔɔ khi pɔι.
48003001	Nɛr Galasι də̃bələ amɛ ka li ninakɛ tɔr? Nɛrɛɛkɛ wι mιɛnι casι Jeju Kirisitii thιr kpa dιι ho nɛr tʋɔr yire.
48003002	Thĩ bɩɛl dιbara hale mι-n ƴaalnι ɩ̃ jι nar: Jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra nι kɔɔ 'lɛ Thu Phuu yaa, ha pɛ thιmιιrraakɛ nι kɔɔ nιnι gι?
48003003	Ãyaal dι nι thʋ̃ də̃bəəl mɛ̃, a ka 'li fʋʋr na Thu Phuu sι na-n ƴaal nɛnɛ̃ nι pɩɩr na anι thɛthɛɛ fãgaa?
48003004	Gι do khaar nι thʋ̃ gaar bʋɔ thale bɛɛ? Dι gι hor khaar khʋʋra gι-n jalna.
48003005	Dι ʋrɛɛkɛ n hana nιnι Thu Phuu, kɛ n cʋɛnι dakha nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ anι thɩ̃thιιn, jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛra gɩ the yaa, ha pɛ thɩmɩɩ nɩɩrra gɩ?
48003006	Mee gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Abɩraham kɔɔ pɛr Thãgba haar dɩɩ do gɛr Thãgba hɩɩn sa wɩɩ tɩɩ sarʋ.”
48003007	Nɩ jɛ gɩ do wɩrɛ hananɩ ha pɛrɛ Thãgbara wɛr dɔ Abɩrahamɩ bɩsãsɔ.
48003008	Mɔ̃ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ kɔɔ 'laanɩ yɩɛ dɩ Thãgba na cʋʋrɛ sor dɩ ga-n hɛl ca kpalala ha pɛrɛra, gɛr gɩ dɩɩ kɔɔ mãa mɩɩrɛ tutugo bʋɔ Abɩrahamna ayɩ: “Fɛr na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ tibil caar fɛʋ na 'lɛ bɔnanɛ.”
48003009	Dɩ mɛ̃ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar n 'lɛ bɔnanɛ na Abɩraham ha pɛdaar.
48003010	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n bɔnɩ dɩ wa-n yɩrna jɔfʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋrɛ, sʋɔn n 'li wer; gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Sʋɔn n 'le tibil wo tibilikɛ na-n hɩnɛnɩ da-n nɩna nũu gɩrɛra fɛʋʋkɛ sɔnɩ jɔfʋ sɛbɛra ga.”
48003011	Wo, tibil bɩɛllakɛ na 'lɛ so hɛllɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra jɔfʋra ga, dɩ sobɔr gɩ, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere wo ayɩ: “Ʋrɛ Thãgba hɛllɔnɩ sor dɩɩ do ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ, ɔr na hana yire.”
48003012	Dɩ jɔfʋ na ha kha dɩkha na ha pɛra', sɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “Ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n cʋɛnɩ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ, a na hana garɛ yire.”
48003013	Kirisiti birse ser sɔ̃ 'lirrə jɔfʋra, gɩdonɩ sɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ firo 'lɛ sʋɔn, gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Sʋɔn gɩ do tibil wo tibilləəkɛ wɩ-n juni kʋkʋ thɩrʋra.”
48003014	Dɩ mɛ̃ bɔnanɛɛkɛ Abɩraham kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ na do dakha ca kpalaada, dɩ Jeju Kirisitira gɩ-n the, dɩ dakha ha pɛrɛra sa 'lɛ Thu Phuukɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛna sɩnɩ.
48003015	Omɩna wei, tibiile mι-n mιι gιrɛ, a tιbιla ƴɛrɛrakɛ ʋlfɛ ʋlfɛrɛ, tibil na hale na puno na phii agιbo a dɛbιrɔ dιkha ga.
48003016	Sι Abιraham ʋlfɛrɛɛle kɔɔ telẽ na ɔɔ məl, ga so ɔɔ məlsɔ dιι ho wι jɔra', sι bιɛl gι so, gιdonɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “afɩ məl”, a thɩɛna gaa Kirisiti gι.
48003017	Nɩ yɛ gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ ɩ̃ so: Nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ 'lini ʋlfɛrɛ, jɔfʋʋkɛ pɩrɔnɩ kpaan yɛna taanã na kpelẽ yʋɔr na puno gi na phii, gɩ do gɛr cʋɛ ʋlfɛrɛɛle dɩɩ kʋkʋʋla'.
48003018	Gɩdonɩ ado jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛ na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sa 'lɛ gɩrɛ Thãgba thɩɩn sarnɩ, ga do ʋlfɛrɛra gɩ the bã, sɩ mee Thãgba kɔɔ ha gɛr Abɩraham dɩɩ do ʋlfɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ.
48003019	Sɩ jɔfʋ anyera gɩ hale? Wɩ pɩrɔrɛ 'laa dɩɩ do sopugo cʋʋrɛ dɔ nɔɔ, phaphapha məlleele n ɩ̃, ʋrɛɛkɛ ʋlfɛrɛɛle kɔɔ telenι; dι jɔfʋʋle thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ kɔɔ gbaan a dʋ thιmιι gʋʋrdaar nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
