48003020	Dι thιmιι gʋʋrdaar na-n hale tιι bιɛlla ga, sι ado Thãgba wer gι, ɔr bιɛl gι.
48003021	Dɩ jɔfʋ n ba kɛ̃kɛrɛnanɛ Thãgbaa ʋlfɛsɔ yaa? Kpɩɩraka'. Ado jɔfʋ kɔɔ hale dɩ wɩ 'laa dɩɩ 'laa yire, ga dor jɔfʋra so hɛllɛ na the bɔɔbɔɔ.
48003022	Sɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ n nɩnanɛ dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ sopugoo nyɔ̃kɔɔ wɩ ha, dɩ mɛ̃ ga dor wɩrɛɛkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar n 'lɛr ʋlfɛrɛ, ga-n the ha pɛrɛraakɛ wɩ hananɩ Jeju Kirisitira.
48003023	Ɔbɔɔkɛ ha pɛrɛ na kɔɔ ɩnɩ pa', jɔfʋ khaɩdara sɩ kɔɔ do, sa-n pɩɛrna ha pɛrɛɛkɛ na yɩranɩ phubi.
48003024	Mɛ̃ jɔfʋ kɔɔ do thɔthɔɔkɛ na thɔɔ sɩnɩ na dana Kirisiti, sor n puno gɩ hɛl sar ha pɛrɛra.
48003025	Dɩ ha pɛrɛ ιnɩ sa ha kha dɩkha na thɔthɔɔdaarɩle 'lo bã.
48003026	Gɩdonɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ Thãgbaa bikona nɩ do ha pɛrɛraakɛ nɩ hananɩ Jeju Kirisitira;
48003027	nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ kpɛɛnɩ nyʋɔnɔ bɩɛl dʋʋrra nakha Kirisiti, Kirisitira nɩ to.
48003028	Juifi dʋʋr na hale dι wιrɛ na dɔnι Juifisɔ waa ga; dee na hale dι waι ga; kuun na hale dι khɛr ga; gɩdonɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛl nɩ do Jeju Kirisitira.
48003029	Dɩ ado Kirisitiida nɩ do, ga dor nɛr dʋɔn Abɩrahamɩ məlsɔ, dɩ thɩ̃ hɩna hanɩ mɔ̃kɛ ʋlfɛrɛ sonɩ.
48004001	Gɩrɛ mɩ sonɩ dʋɔn wɔɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ thɩ̃ hɩn donɩ bɩsaan, gɛr aa-n har kpɩɩ na dea', sɩɩ dorakɛ ɔr dʋɔn kɔ̃tɩn thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra;
48004002	sɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ n hɩnɛɛnɩ na kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ a-n ha, phaphapha bɔɔkɛ thɩrɛ pɛrnɩ n dã.
48004003	Sɛrɛ dakha mɛna gɩ ha sar, ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ honɩ bɩsana, sɩ kɔɔ dor dea dɩɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ bɔ taa dɩɩra', kɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ tinəneeda.
48004004	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ bɔɔ kɔɔ danɩ, Thãgba kɔɔ thɔnanɛ ɔɔ Bikuun, khɛr kɔɔ kɔnaa, jɔfʋ hʋɛra wɩ kɔɔ kʋ̃ɔ,
48004005	dɩ mɛ̃ a na puno na birse wɩrɛ hanɩ jɔfʋ hʋɛra, gɩ do nɔɔ a gba sɩ sɩ do ɔɔ bikuunsɔ.
48004006	Dɩ gɩdonɩ bikona ha nɩ, Thãgba thʋɔn ɔɔ Bikuuni Thu dɩ lõ anɩ hara da-n wɩɩ: Aba; kɩrʋ dʋɔn: Thɩrɛ.
48004007	Mɛ̃ gɩ fa do dee bã, sɩ bikuun fɩ do, dɩ ado bikuun fɩ do, fɛr dʋɔn thɩ̃ hɩn, dɩɩ do Thãgba dɔ nɔɔ.
48004008	Mamara na kɔɔ jɩnɩ Thãgba ga, nɩ kɔɔ dor dea dɩkhasɔraakɛ na dɔnɩ thãgba ga.
48004009	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ nɩ jɩrɛ Thãgba, dɩrakɛ Thãgba ka kɔɔ jɩ nɩ, sɩ mɔ̃ gɩ fʋ dɩ nɩ bir kɛr na-n bir dɩɩrɛraalera na-n taanɩ bʋɔa', kɛ n kɔnɩ bʋɔ; anye hale dɩ nɩ ƴaal nɩ birə dɔ gar dea wo?
48004010	Nɩ hananɛ pərre wi hɩɩnɛnasɔ, na porasɔra, na bɔɔsɔra, na yɛnasɔra.
48004011	Maar fʋ mɛr dɩ agakpaana ɩ̃ thɔ̃ɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ donɩ jɔɔ nɛrɛra ga dor mɔlɔ gɩ.
48004012	Mɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr omɩna, nɩ hana mɔ̃kɛ mɩ hanɩ, gɩdonɩ mɛrɛ dakha mɩ har mɔ̃kɛ nɩ hanɩ.
48004013	Na kɔɔ cʋʋ mɩ puure fɩɩʋraka'; nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ caca bɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, ɩ̃ tomɩ sɩ kɔɔ dɔ nɔɔ.
48004014	Ɩ̃ kho kɔɔ do narɛ nɩwɛ, sɩ na kɔɔ ƴʋɔn ma', ma kɔɔ yaa nɩ dakha woa'; nɩ kɔɔ tee mer dɩ ɩ̃ ho Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu a ho Jeju Kirisiti.
48004015	Kana ga kãka caalera jal gɩrɛ kper? Gɩdonɩ mɩ-n mɩɩrɛ anɩda ayɩ: Ado hʋɛ kɔɔ harrɛra ga dor na kɔɔ tire anɩ yi a na ha mɩ.
48004016	Mɩ debire do nar lãlaardaar nɛnɛ̃ sobɔrraakɛ mɩ-n so narnɩ yaa?
48004017	Gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ ca gele tibil ca wele hana narnɩ, ga do gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ bʋɔ ga, wɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n lea sɩ kha nɩ bir nɩ ma wɩ.
48004018	Gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ hananɛ wer bɔɔ fɛʋ thɩɛnaakɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ, gɩ bɔrɛ, sɩ ga-n do bɔɔkɛ mɩ hanɩ kha na nɛrɛ dɩbara ga.
48004019	Ɩ̃ bɩsãsɔ wei, anɩ wal birə gɩrɛ fʋ mɩ wo, phaphapha Kirisiti n jɩɩ ɩɩr anɩ bɩnɔ.
48004020	Mɩ narra a ho wɩ yɛ nɛnɛ̃ ɩ̃ birə hana anɩ pa a jɛ mɔ̃ ma mɩɩnɩ, gɩdonɩ ma thʋ̃ jɩ gɩrɛ ma cʋʋnι anιdarara bã.
48004021	Nɩ sɔ mar, nɛrkɛra n ƴaalɛnɩ nɩ birə hana jɔfʋra, na nɩ gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonaa?
48004022	Mee gɩ kherere ayɩ: Abɩraham kɔɔ hananɛ bikona yenyɔ, bιɛl do deekhɛrι bi, bιɛl do wa khɛrι bi.
48004023	Sι deekhɛrι bi wer, birə gι dι wι kɔ̃ mɔ̃ wɛ n kɔnι; sι wa khɛr wer, Thãgbaa ʋlfɛ bi a kɔ̃.
48004024	Thɩ̃ɛɛle sokpaa gι, gιdonι khɛra yenyɔɔle n nɛna nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛrɛ yenyɔ. Agaar n nɛna mɔ̃ ʋlfɛ bιɛl hanι, kɛ dɔnι Sιnaι gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔda, ɔr kɔna dee bi.
48004025	Gιdonι Agaar hʋɔn Sιnaι gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔkɛ hanι Arabι dιιra, a hona dakha nɛnɛ̃ Jerujalɛmkɛ gιrɛ, kɛ hanι dee paar na ɔɔ bιsãsɔ.
48004026	Sι ƴũ Jerujalɛm waʋ gι, dι ɔr dɔ asι nι.
48004027	Gιdonι gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Na kãkanɛ fɛr kʋ̃ʋbʋʋkɛ na kɔɔ kɔnanɩ bə', mana na bɛna hulẽbe, fɛrɛɛkɛ wallɛ na kɔɔ fʋnɩ kpɩɩa', gɩdonɩ khɛrɩkɛ wɩ faanɩɩ bisɔ jɔrɛ ka, a ka jɔ khɛr ʋrɛ hananɩ kuun.”
48004028	Sɩ ado nɛr wɛ omɩna, nɛr dʋɔn ʋlfɛ bɩsana Ɩjakɩɩ kha.
48004029	Dɩ mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ hanɩ dɩɩ do biikɛra wɩ kɔnɩ wɛɛ kha n kɔɔ kpoone ʋrɛraakɛ wɩ kɔnɩ dɩɩ do Thu Phuu pa gɩ the, mɛna gɩ ha gɩrɛ nĩ.
48004030	Sɩ anye Thãgbaa sɛbɛ so ayɩ: “Wea deekhɛr na ɔɔ bikuun a faa, gɩdonɩ deekhɛrɩ bi na do thɩ̃ hɩna', sɩ wa khɛrɩ bi na dɔ thɩ̃ hɩn.”
48004031	Gɛr gɩ omɩna wei, sa do deekhɛrɩ bisɔa', sɩ wa khɛrɩ bisɔ sɩ do.
48005001	Wa dʋʋrra Kirisiti kɔɔ birse si, gɛr gɩ nɩ fɔ gɩ ma, na-n do dee dʋʋr n bir gɩ 'li ni bã.
48005002	Nɩ hɩnɛ mɛr Pol mɩ so narɛ ayɩ, ado na kur khʋ̃ʋ ga dor Kirisiti na taa nɩ bʋɔ bã.
48005003	Dɩ mɩ-n kpãkpãa narɛ wo ayɩ, ado tibil kur khʋ̃ʋ, jɔfʋ ntɛ yɩ ɩna-n hɩɩnɛ fɛʋ.
48005004	Nɩ leere na Kirisiti nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ sor n hɛla nar jɔfʋ cʋʋrɛra, nι 'leere dakha Thãgbaa bɔ jι.
48005005	Ado se wer so hɛl nũ pɛrɛ sι-n pιɛr, kɛ Thu Phuu na cʋʋnι dι sa 'lɛ ha pɛrɛra.
48005006	Gιdonι a fι ha Jeju Kirisitira a fι kurre khʋ̃ʋ yo, a fa kur khʋ̃a yo, ga-n cʋʋ thɩ̃a', sι ha pɛrɛɛkɛ hananι naʋʋkɛ n cʋɛnι thɩ̃ɛ, gɛr dɔ thɩ̃ɛ.
48005007	Nι kɔɔ car waa gel, sι amɛ jιlɛ nι a pιɛr nι na-n nι sobɔr nũə?
48005008	Kpιɛr ca gele na the ʋrɛraakɛ kɔɔ wɛ nιna'.
48005009	Tabιιr fιιʋ n cʋʋrɛ buru mɩ̃ boloo fɛʋ dιι bʋ̃.
48005010	Mι hana narɛ ha pɛrɛ Kɔ̃tιnna, dι na hana kpιɛr kpιa', sι ʋrɛɛkɛ nyanyaanɛ nιnι ado a ha mɔnakɛ, sι sor na heenuune.
48005011	Sι ado me wer omɩna, ado ɩ̃ Thãgba thɩmɩɩ mɩɩra mɩ yɩ wa-n kuro khʋ̃ʋ, anyera ma-n yɩ kpoore 'lo? Gιdonι Kirisitii kʋkʋ thιr thιmιιkɛ n dɔnι nɛ baradaa, gι bure mɛ̃.
48005012	Dι wιrɛra n pιɛrnι nyanyaanɛ anι thɩ̃thιιn wι yιra kuro kpɔ khorr.
48005013	Omιna wei, wa dʋʋrra Thãgba kɔɔ we nι, sι na-n gba wa dʋʋrra a phiro sι na cʋʋ gιrɛɛkɛ anι tibil do pa n ƴaalna', sι nι ka dɔ kha dea bιɛlbιɛl naʋra.
48005014	Gιdonι jɔfʋ fɛʋ, thιmιι nɔ bιɛllaakɛ gι ha ayι: “Fa-n na afι 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃kɛ fι-n nanι afιbara.”
48005015	Sι ado nι-n dʋɔnɛ kha a na phʋʋna khasɔ, na-n jιɛ hιιn na-n kʋɛ khasɔa koe.
48005016	Gɛr gι dι ɩ̃ so nar ayι: Na-n jala mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuu n so narnι, ga cʋʋ nɛr dι na cʋʋ gιrɛ anι tibil do pa n ƴaalna'.
48005017	Gιdonι gιrɛ tibili tibil do pa n ƴaalnι, ga-n 'li kha fιιʋrakɛ na gιrɛ Thu Phuu n ƴaalna'; dι gιrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n ƴaalnι, ga-n 'li kha fιιʋrakɛ na gιrɛ tibili tibil do pa n ƴaalna'; wɛr yenyɔ wι-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ kha, dι gɛr gι na-n puno na cʋʋ gιrɛɛkɛ nι pɛrnι haara'.
48005018	Sι ado Thu Phuuda nι-n pɛ nũu jɔfʋ na puno na'.
48005019	Dι gιrɛra tibili tibil do pa n cʋʋnɩ gɩ yɩrrɛ gbelẽ gbelẽ, gɛr ha gɩrɛ: Bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ, thɩ̃ bise cʋʋrɛ, dakhaba cʋʋrɛ,
48005020	thɩl jir, dɔɔrɛ, tɩɩ laarɛ, kɩla, gbugi, nĩkhii, dɩbara na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ, dɩɩdɩɩ leere, thʋ̃ kha,
48005021	ha pɩɛrɛ, ta laarɛ, gbõgolõ dɩko khor, na yɛ̃ thĩsɔɔkɛ n hɔnɩ kha na gɩrɛra. Mɩ maanɛ dɩ ma-n so nar gɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛra mɩ kɔɔ sonɩ, dɩ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ wa lõ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dʋɔa'.
48005022	Sɩ beekɛ Thu Phuu n senɩ dʋɔn: Naʋ, daʋ, ha ɩɩ, ha fʋrɛ, ha bulo fɩlɛ, bɔ cʋʋrɛ, sobɔ cʋʋrɛ,
48005023	hɛlɛlɛ fιlɛ, dιbara fʋrɛ; jɔfʋ na hale dιι pιɛr ga thɩ̃sɔɔka'.
48005024	Dι wιrɛ hanι Jeju Kirisitira wι gbaar tibili tibil do pa na gιrɛ na-n kʋɔnι thue kpãkpalã ga, na dakha ɔɔ ƴaal a kpa kʋkʋ thιrʋra.
48005025	Dι Thu Phuu donι ʋrɛ n hana sιnι yire, sa-n ιrɛ mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuurə n so sarnι.
48005026	Sa-n ƴaal mɔlɔ i ka thɩ̃ɛ ga-n ιna sar nãbɛɛrɛ, sa-n gba kha gbugisɔa'.
48006001	Omιna wei, ado nι yι tibilikɛ hanι sopugo cʋʋrɔ, nɛrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnι Thu Phuudara nι naarɛɛ na hɛlɛlɛ fιlɛ, sι jιɛ hιιn afιbara a mɛ̃ gaa fa 'lɛr fifiləle fer.
48006002	Na-n dea kha heendaasɔ, thale dɔ Kirisitii jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛ.
48006003	Ado tibil na kpɩɛr dɩ ɩnɩ dor thɩ̃ɛ sɩɩ do aa do thɩ̃a', dɩbara a-n fɩɩl.
48006004	Tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl n jʋrɛ awɩ thɛthɛɛ thɔ̃ a na hɩnɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ tibil na hana ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ məbida dɩbara, sɩ a na-n too na barana haanɩda ga;
48006005	gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ telenenɩ tibil, dɔ a na-n hɩɩn gɛr.
48006006	Dɔ ʋrɛ wɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ na-n bɔna ʋrɛ n dɩrɛɛnɩ na ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔ fɛʋʋkɛ a hananɩ.
48006007	Na-n fɩɩl dɩbara ga; wa-n ɓoɓoro Thãgbara ga, gɩrɛ tibil n diirni gɛrra a na kha.
48006008	Ʋrɛɛkɛ direni dɩɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ tibili tibil do pa n ƴaalnɩ, tibili tibil do padara a na kha gɩ do kʋɛrɛ, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ direni dɩɩ do Thu Phuudaa gɩ, Thu Phuudaara a na kha gɩ do yire khorr.
48006009	Sa-n do nyɛ̃ɛ n khiir si bɔ cʋʋrɛra ga, gιdonι ado bɔɔ dã sa khar ado sa kɔɔ pɛr dokhʋʋra'.
48006010	Mɛ̃ gι nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ sι yιnι hʋɛ, sa-n cʋɛ tιbιla fɛʋ bɔɔ, sι cacaca wιrɛ dɔnι ha pɛdara.
48006011	Nι hιnɛ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ khera nar sɛbɛ beekɛ gbõgbõo na ɩ̃ nyɛ̃.
48006012	Wιrɛ n ƴaalɛnι i bɔ wer gιrɛraakɛ tibil yinə n yιnι, wɛr n yιrana nι nι kuro khʋ̃ʋ, kιrʋ dʋɔn kpoore wa-n ƴaal Kirisitii kʋkʋ thιrdara ga.
48006013	Gιdonι welela yɛnιnakɛ khʋ̃ʋ ιnι kur, sι wa-n hιιn jɔfʋa', sι wι-n ƴaalɛ nι kuro khʋ̃ʋ wι yι hʋɛ wa-n məbi jιιnnaale wι pɛ narnι tomιrra.
48006014	Sι ado merra wer, thɩ̃ kpιι na hale ma-n məbironi saagado asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii kʋkʋ thιrdara gaaga. Kʋkʋ thιrʋra dʋɔn gιrɛ cʋɛnι dιι do thιιkɛɛda do marɛ thɩ̃ khire dι mɛrɛ dakha mι khire gιrɛraakɛ dɔnι thιιkɛɛda.
48006015	Gιdonι a fι kurre khʋ̃ʋ yo, a fa kur khʋ̃a yo, ga-n cʋʋ thɩ̃a', gιrɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ɛ gɛr dʋɔn tιι pha dʋʋr.
48006016	Wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na tuonni dιιrɛɛkɛ kɛ dɔnι Thãgbaa Ɩjιrayɛlιda, Thãgba na-n hana wι ha ιι a na-n dɔna wι dakha bʋɔ.
48006017	Nɛnɛ̃ dιphã tibil na-n thʋ̃ na pɛ mar nιwɛra bã, Jejuu i dɔ nɔɔ mι 'lɛrɔnι pɔnaakɛ ɩ̃ tomιra.
48006018	Omιna wei, asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra. Amɛn.
49001001	Mɛr Polιkɛ dɔnι Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha tιι phuusɔɔkɛ dɔnι sobɔ omιnaakɛ Jeju Kirisiti hιnι, dι wι ha Efɛjι.
49001002	Thãgba asι Thι na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιn n hana nι ha ιι a jɛ nɩ dakha bʋɔra.
49001003	Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii Thɩ hɩna khɩɩrɛ, kɛ kɔɔ bɔna sɩnɩ na bɔna caar dɩɩdɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ thudaa, kɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ dιι do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
49001004	Thale Thãgba phiir si dιι do Jeju Kirisitii pa gι the, sι aa kɔɔ ti thιιkɛ pa' ayι, sι pho a 'lea dι paar ɔɔ ƴɛra. Ɔɔ naʋra
49001005	a kɔɔ mãa phiir sar dι sa dʋʋraa bιsana, gι do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ daaraanɩ haar dɩ ƴaal,
49001006	sɩ puno sa-n khɩsʋʋ ɔɔ nɔ kpaa bɔ jɩ hananaakɛra a kɔɔ jɩ sɩnɩ dɩɩ do ɔɔ Bikuunikɛ a nanɩ dɔ nɔɔ.
49001007	Ɔrra sɩ 'lɛ birsere na sopugo faarɛ dɩɩ the ɔɔ tɔmɩna, a ha mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ bɔ jɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ
49001008	ɔr Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ sɩnɩ jɔɔ hanɩ, a hanana sɩ kpɛsɛrɛ na jɩɩr fɛʋ.
49001009	Ɔr cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sɩ jɩ ɔɔ tuurikɛ keranɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ ƴaal bɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ hananɩ ɔɔ hara kɛkɛkɛ,
49001010	gɛr dʋɔn ado bɔɔ dã ɩna gbɛbɩrɛ gɩrɛ fɛʋ hanɩ ƴũ na thɩɩra dɩ ga do bɩɛl Kirisiti n do gar yʋʋ.
49001011	Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ phiir si dɩ sa ha kpɩɩ mɔ̃ a kɔɔ maanɩ ƴaalɛ, gɩdonɩ ɔr n cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ ga-n ha mɔ̃ a-n ƴaalnɩ gɩ hana,
49001012	sɩ puno sa-n khɩsʋʋ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ hanana, sɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ kɔɔ kʋlɛnɩ ƴɩɛ a hana nũ pɛrɛ Kirisitira.
49001013	Nɛrɛ dakha nɩ kɔɔ pɛrɛ haar ɔrra ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ sobɔ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ hananι taarɛ, dι ɔrra dakha dɔ nɔɔ dι Thãgba dʋ nar jιιnιkɛ dɔnι Thu Phuukɛ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛnι ιna ' laarɛ,
49001014	ɔr dɔ barã paar gιrɛraakɛ sa 'lɛnι, a cʋʋ sɛr dɩ sɩ jɩ tue dɩ Thãgba na taarɛ dɩphã waa vʋ̃ʋ wιrɛ a hɩnɩ, wɩ puno wɩ do wɩrɛ na-n khɩsaanɩ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ hanana.
49001015	Gɛr gɩ mɛrɛ dakha mɔ̃kɛ mɩ nɩɛnɩ anɩ thɩmɩɩ ha pɛrɛraakɛ nɩ hananɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnna, na anɩ naakɛ nɩ-n nanɩ tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋ.
49001016	Ma-n pɩr Thãgba khɩɩrɛ kpɩɩ anɩdara ga. Mɩ-n wer anɩ i dι ma-n bιɛlna
49001017	asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι Thιrɛɛkɛ hιnanι i dʋbιrɛ, a hana nι Thu Phuu a na-n ha nι kpɛsɛrɛ a na-n nιnana nι nι jιι jιι;
49001018	a phuo ni dakha yire nι jι mɔ̃ nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ we narnι hanι, nι jιna mɔ̃ ɔɔ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ ɓɔ̃ɔkɛ a thιιnnι ɔɔ tιι phusɔra hanι,
49001019	nι jιna dakha ɔɔ fãga kʋkʋʋkɛ hanιle sɛr ha pɛdaraa ha, ga fãga caalera wabanι thale;
49001020	gɛr a kɔɔ ιιrna Kirisiti dι the khirera a cʋʋnaa dι too gιrɛ ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra le Thãgbaa dʋɔ,
49001021	a kəə fãgadarara fɛʋ, na punodarara fɛʋ, na dakpɛna yʋʋsɔra fɛʋ, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔra fɛʋ, a kəəna thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩɛna fɛʋʋkɛ hananɩ ire dɩ wɩ we, ga do nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛ gɩ dɩbara ga, sɩ bɔɔraakɛ na ɩnanɩ dakha.
49001022	Dɩ Thãgbara gbaar thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ jəəro nɛɛ, a pɩɛraarɛ dɩ do yʋʋ we gbɛbɩdarara.
49001023	We gbɛbɩdarara dɔ ɔɔ tomɩɩkɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ hironi phi ɔrkɛ henɩ thɩɩkɛra a gbana ƴũ koo.
49002001	Anɩ dɩ pa na anɩ sopugo dor nɔɔ dɩ nɩ kɔɔ khi mamara;
49002002	dabɔɔlera nɩ kɔɔ ha garnɩ dɩ na-n kpaan na fɩlɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ thɩɩkɛɛda, dɩ na-n nɩ nũu ʋrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩn fãgadarasɔraakɛ dɔnɩ thudaakɛ hanɩ jɩɛra le ƴũ, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ n dɔnanɩ gɩrɛ nũ nʋʋrdara thɔma.
49002003	Sɛrɛ fɛʋ dakha thalera sɩ kɔɔ ha dɩ sa-n kɔɔ ɩɩr mɔ̃kɛ asɩ tibil do pa n ƴaalnɩ, dɩ sa-n cʋʋna dakha gɩrɛ n kɔnɩ asɩ tomɩ na asɩ kpɩɛr thue, dɩ asɩ ti parakɛ Thãgbaa nĩkhi too sɩ too ɩkhasɔɔ kha.
49002004	Sɩ Thãgbaakɛ ɔɔ bɔ dona na wabɩnɩ kpãkpalã ga, na ɔɔ naʋ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ a kɔɔ na sɩnɩ,
49002005	sɩɩ dorakɛ sɛr dɔ wɩrɛ kɔɔ khenɩ dɩɩ do asɩ dɩ pa dɔ nɔɔ a bire ha sɩ yire na Kirisiti. Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ nɩ 'lɛ taarɛ.
49002006	A kɔɔ ɩɩr sɛr kha dɩ sɩ gbɛbɩ too Thãgbaa dʋɔ nakha Kirisiti, dɩɩ the asɩ bɩɛl dora na Jeju Kirisiti.
49002007	Gɩ do nɔɔ a nɩna bɔɔraakɛ n ɩnanɩ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ bɔ jɩ thʋnɩ wabɩ, dɩɩ the bɔɔraakɛ a bɔ sarnɩ dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
49002008	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩra nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛ taarɛ dɩɩ the ha pɛrɛra, ga do anɩ pa gɩ tha', Thãgbaa khaarda gɩ.
49002009	Məbi paar na ha liir tibil n məbiroə', gɩdonɩ ga do anɩ dɩkha cʋʋra gι tha'.
49002010	Gιdonι sɛr dɔ Thãgbaa nyɛ̃ thɔ̃; a kɔɔ ti ser dιι do Jeju Kirisitii pa gι the, sa-n cʋɛ thɔ̃ bʋɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ maanι gbɛbιrɛ sa-n cʋɛ.
49002011	Gɛr gι nι jɛna gιrɛ nɩ kɔɔ donɩ mamara, nɛr kɔɔ dɔ ca kpalaakɛ Juifisɔ n hɩɩnnɩ mɔ̃ na donɩ khʋ̃ kurdara ga, sɩɩ do mɔ̃ wι donι khʋ̃ kurdara jιιn gιιkɛ tibil nyɛ̃ɛ pɛrnι.
49002012	Ɔbɔɔraalera na kɔɔ hana Kirisita', na kɔɔ hana lõ paar Ɩjιrayɛldaraa thɩ̃thιιna', nι kɔɔ dor kpakpala nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛrɛraakɛ kɔɔ ʋlfɛnɛnι, na kɔɔ hana nũ pɛra', na kɔɔ hana Thãgba thιιraaka'.
49002013	Sι nɛnɛ̃ dιphã nɛrkɛ kɔɔ hʋnɔnɛnι mamara, Kirisitii tɔmɩ̃ cʋʋ nɛr dι nι tɔ wɔrɔ̃ gιrɛ, dιι the anι bιɛl dora na Jeju Kirisiti.
49002014	Gιdonι ɔr dʋɔn asι ha ie, ɔrkɛ cʋɛnι Juifisɔ na ca kpala dι wι do bιɛl, mɔ̃ a wιɛlnι laarɛɛkɛ dɔnι gʋʋkɛ lea wɩnɩ kha.
49002015	Ɔɔ tomɩ a gba a kʋkʋʋlna jɔfʋ na gιrɛ jɔfʋ n yιnι foo gι cʋɛ, na sɔsɔɔkɛ gι hananι, a cʋʋrɛ mɛ̃ gɩ do nɔɔ caar yenyɔɔle n gbɛbɩ wɩ do tɩɩ pha bɩɛl, gɩ do thale dɔ ha ɩɩ a pɛrnɩ.
49002016	Ɔɔ khi kʋkʋ thɩrʋra a kʋna laarɛ, a cʋʋna dakha caar yenyɔ dɩ wɩ bir kũu kha na Thãgba a do tomɩ bɩɛl.
49002017	A kɔɔ ɩnɛ a mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ ha iedaa nɛrɛraakɛ hʋnɔnɛnɩ na Thãgba, na wɩrɛraakɛ wɔrɔnɛnɩ.
49002018	Ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ sɛrɛ bɩɛlbɩɛl yɩ lõ paar Thɩrɛra na Thu Phuu bɩɛl.
49002019	Gɛr gɩ dɩphã na do kpakpala na hʋ ka bã, sɩ bɩɛl nɩ do na tɩɩ phuusɔ a dona Thãgbaa cɔ too.
49002020	Nɛr dɔ cʋɔrɩkɛ mɛnɩ, sɩ thɔ̃thɔna na Thãgba tukɩr tidara kɔɔ kpɛa gʋʋ ɓo, dɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɛthɛ dɔ go tɩ bokaar.
49002021	Bɩɛl dʋʋr na ɔr thɛthɛ na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ cʋɔrra fɛʋ na cõcool na khɔ̃ a na do cɔ phuu Kɔ̃tɩnna.
49002022	Bɩɛl dʋʋrrara na ɔr wɩ gba nɩ a ɓaan a gbɛbɩ mι dι nι do cʋɔr Thãgbara, kɛ Thu Phuu n cɔrɔnι.
49003001	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dι mɛr Polιkɛ dɔnι khaɩdaar Jeju Kirisitii sora dɩɩ do nɛr ca kpala dɔ nɔɔ, n bɩɛl Thãgba dɩ ma-n pɛ nar.
49003002	Mɩ pɛrɛ haar nɩ nɩɛrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba pɛ marnɩ thɔma dɩ ma-n cʋʋ nɛrɛra, dɩɩ do ɔɔ bɔ jɩra gɩ the.
49003003	Thãgba kɔɔ nɛ mar thɩ̃ɛ a cʋʋ mɩ dɩ ɩ̃ jɩ thɩ̃ gbulikɛ keranɩ, gɛr ha gɩrɛ mɩ kherenɩ a cʋɩ nar gbe;
49003004	dɩ mɔ̃ nɩ-n hɩɩnnɩ sɛbɛɛkɛ na punone na jɩ dɩ mɩ jɩɛ jɩ Kirisitii thɩ̃ gbulilera.
49003005	Bɔɔkɛ kɔɔ kanɩ mamara tɩbɩla na kɔɔ jɩ thɩ̃ gbulikɛ mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuu nɩna gɩnɩ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar phusɔra na ɔɔ tukɩr tidarara ga.
49003006	Gɛr dɔ mɔ̃ ca kpala na bulni kha na Juifisɔ gɩrɛ wɩ hananɩ, a na debi dakha a na do tomɩ bɩɛlɩ ɓãɓã na wɛr, a na bulnə kha Thãgbaa ʋlfɛɛkɛ tibil na 'lɛnɩ Jeju Kirisitira gɩ do tutugo bʋɔra gɩ the,
49003007	kɛ mɩ doronɩ gɩrɛ thɔ̃thɔn dɩɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ khaardaakɛ Thãgba ha mɩnɩ ɔɔ fãgara hanɩ, sɩ dɩɩ do ɔɔ bɔ jɩra gɩ the.
49003008	Mɛrkɛ dɔnɩ dabuu a jɔ tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋ, sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ mɛr bʋɔra a pɛ mar ma-n mɩa ca kpala tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnι Kirisitii thɩ̃ ɓɔ̃ɔkɛ na hanι mιɛrɛra ga,
49003009	ɩ̃ cʋɛ tιbιla fɛʋ wι jιι yι mɔ̃ thɩ̃ gbullə yιrnι, gιrɛ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ Tidaar kɔɔ maanι kerre kɛkɛkɛ.
49003010	Mɛ̃ dιphã we gbɛbιdara na cʋʋ fãgadara na punodara Thãgbaa dʋɔ dι wa jι Thãgbaa kpɛsɛɛkɛ jʋɔnɔnι.
49003011	Thãgba cʋʋrɛ mɛ̃ dιι nιna ɔɔ kpιɛrιkɛ dɔnι khorrdaakɛ yιranι dιι do asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira gι the,
49003012	kɛ sι yιrɔnι hʋɛ na ha pɛrɛɛkɛ sι hananaanι a na ba wɔrɔna Thãgba na 'lar.
49003013	Mɛ̃ gι mι-n bιɛl nɛr na-n do nyɛ̃ɛ n khiir ni bɔ gaarɛraakɛ mι-n yιnι anι sora ga, anι dabɔ ga kɛr na do.
49003014	Gɛr dɔ kιrʋ dι ma-n gulẽga Thιrɛɛ ƴɛra,
49003015	kɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanι thιιra na ƴũ n 'lɛrnι ire,
49003016	dι a na gba ɔɔ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ ɓɔ̃ a cʋʋna nι nι 'lɛ fãga gι jɔr anι hara, gι do ɔɔ Thu Phuurə gι the;
49003017	Kirisiti n tɔɔ dakha anι hara gι the ha pɛrɛra, nι puno nι gɔ nɛɛ gι hulõ naʋra;
49003018	nι puno na-n jι na tιι phuusɔ fɛʋ mɔ̃ Kirisitii naʋ pɛrnι, a gbaanna, a hulona, a gbaanna dakha ƴũ;
49003019	nι jιι jιna ɔɔ naʋʋkɛ kanι jιιr fɛʋ, nι puno nι hi phi na Thãgbaa hi fɛʋ.
49003020	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananι punone dι cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛ, dɩɩ do ɔɔ fãgaakɛ n dɔnɩ thɔma asɩ hara gɩ-n the, a-n cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ jɔ gɩrɛ fɛʋ sɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ na sɩ-n kpɩɛrnɩ;
49003021	ɔɔ i n dʋbarɔ we gbɛbɩdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ, gɩ do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the. Amɛn.
49004001	Gɛr gɩ mɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr, mɛrkɛ dɔnɩ khaɩdaar Kɔ̃tɩnɩ sora, na-n ɩrɛ ga-n mɩɛ kha na werɩkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ we nɩnɩ.
49004002	Nɩ jɔ dɩbara, a hana hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ, a hanana dakha ha fʋrɛ. Na-n fɔ kha haar bɩɛlbɩɛl na naʋ.
49004003	Na-n gbuoro yʋʋ Thu Phuu bɩɛl do n hale gɩ too anɩ pa, gɩ do lidaakɛ dɔnɩ ha ɩɩkɛ le nɩnɩ dɔ nɔɔ.
49004004	Tomɩ bɩɛl hale, na Thu Phuu bɩɛl, mɔ̃kɛ nũ pɛ bɩɛl hanɩle dakha kɛ Thãgba we narnɩ.
49004005	Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl dɩbara haanle, na ha pɛ bɩɛl, na yɔ kpɛɛ bɩɛl,
49004006	na Thãgba bɩɛl, kɛ dɔnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ Thɩ, ɔr kəəne thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ pɛnɩ paar fɛʋ, a har dakha sɛrɛ fɛʋʋ bɩnɔ.
49004007	Sɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl 'lɛr bɔ jɩ khaardaa dɩɩ do asɩda, mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti n 'laanɩ jɔɔ dɩ ha sɩ.
49004008	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sonɩ ayɩ: “Mɔ̃ a-n kɔɔ jʋʋnnɩ ƴũ, a khɩɩrɛ dea a jʋʋnna, a har tɩbɩla dakha khaardaa.”
49004009	A jʋʋnɛɛ kιr dʋɔn mɔ̃? Mee gι nιnanɛ a kɔɔ gbune a dã thɩ thɛrɛɛ ɓo.
49004010	Ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ gbunoni ɔr thɛthɛra jʋnɛ a kəə thãgbara ƴũ fɛʋ, dι mɛ̃ ga do ɔr he thιιkɛra a gbana ƴũ koo.
49004011	Ɔr pιɛr ιkhasɔ wι dɔ thɔ̃thɔna, ιkhasɔ n do Thãgba tukιr tidara, ιkhasɔ n do tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι mιιdara, ιkhasɔ n do khɛkhɛ na dιιrdara,
49004012	gι do nɔɔ tιι phuusɔ n gbɛbιrι wι 'li wa-n jιι cʋʋ ɔɔ thɔ̃, gι cʋʋ dakha Kirisitii tomɩ gɩ khɔ̃ ga-n pɛr,
49004013	phaphapha sɛrɛ fɛʋ n do bɩɛl ha pɛdaara, na Thãgbaa Bikuuni jɩra, sɩ khɔ̃ sɩ bɩ̃, sɩ mãkhana Kirisitiikɛ dananɩ thu;
49004014	dɩ mɛ̃ sa do bɩsana 'lo, dɩ dɩɩrɛɛkɛ n phʋnanɩ jɛ khaa na cʋʋ sɩ sa-n kpaar baba ga; dɩɩrɛɛle tɩɩ fɩɩl tɩbɩlaa pa gɩ the, kɛ n gbaannɩ fɩɩlɛ dɩ wɩ cʋʋna tɩbɩla wɩ lona hʋ puurə.
49004015	Sɩ sobɔ mɩɩrɛ na naʋ sa ka na khɔnɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra ʋrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ yʋʋ, a thɩɛna gaa Kirisiti gɩ.
49004016	Ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ tomɩ ɓaanʋsɔ dɩɩdɩɩ n coor kha a do bɩɛl dɩɩ the ƴɔɔpasɔraalera tomɩrra n hananɩ, mɛ̃ gɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tomɩ ɓaanʋ dɩɩdɩɩlera n donɩ awɩ thɔ̃ mɔ̃kɛ gɩ teenanɩ, tomɩrra koo n khʋɔn dɩ ga-n pɛr na naʋ.
49004017	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n sonɩ dɩ ɩ̃ bo dɩ ma-n kpãkpaanɔ mɔ̃ mɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda dʋɔn wɔɔ: Na-n hana fɩlɛ 'lo a ho thɩldaraakɛ hananɩ mɔlɔ kpɩɛra'.
49004018	Awɩ kpɩɛr pa gɩ birəre, wa hana Thãgbaa yiikɛ a-n 'laana', dɩ gele awɩ kpɩɛr 'leeraakɛ wɩ hananɩ na awɩ ha dibirə gɩ the.
49004019	Awɩ puu cʋʋ na-n thʋ wɩ haar fɩɩʋraka'; wɩ gbaar dɩbara a faa dakhaba cʋʋrɛra, dɩ wa-n cʋʋna thɔ̃ bisesɔ fɛʋʋkɛ n kɔ wɩnɩ thue.
49004020	Sɩ nɛrɛ, ga do thale gɩ dɩɩr nɩ Kirisitii pa ga.
49004021	Sɩ mee mɩ pɛrɛ haar nɩ nɩɛrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ mɔ̃ ɔɔda mɩɩnɩ, dɩ wɩ dɩɩr nɛr sobɔrɩkɛ hanɩ Jejura,
49004022	gɛr dʋɔn a thɩɛna gaa dɔ nɩ faa cʋʋ pa tɩ̃ɩkɛ nɩ kɔɔ hananɩ mamara, kɛ dɔnɩ tɩɩ tɩ̃ dʋʋrιkɛ hananι thɩ̃ ƴaal kpãkpãa kheuukɛ na-n hiennə', dιι tʋɔ dι ga-n jalna kʋɛ paar.
49004023	Dɔ nι debi nι do daphaa haarra na kpιɛrɛra.
49004024	Nι tɔ tιι pha dʋʋrιkɛ Thãgba tini da-n hʋʋ fιl sarrɛra na phurrəəkɛ thɛnι sobɔrra.
49004025	Gɛr gι dɔ nι faa sõsor sι nɛrɛ fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl na-n mιι gιrɛ dɔnι sobɔr 'walãkha tibillə, gιdonι tomι ɓãasɔ sι do a dona tomι bιɛl.
49004026	A nĩkhii fʋ nι na-n cʋʋ sopugoə'; na-n do wire n lõ sι nĩkhii n cι nara',
49004027	dι na-n faa Satã a yι lõ paara'.
49004028	Ʋrɛɛkɛ dʋɔnnι yudaar a na-n yu bã, sι a ka na dɔ thɔ̃ bʋɔ na ɔɔ nyɛ̃ a hanana dakha gɩrɛ a na-n 'laanɩ wιrɛraakɛ thɩ̃ɛ n ɓɔrnι.
49004029	Na-n do thιmιι puu bιɛllakɛ na-n the anι nɔa', sι na-n mιa thιmιι bʋɔ tιbιlala mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ ha warnι gι cʋʋ wι wι khɔ̃ wa-n pɛr, gι dɔ thιmιaakɛ na bʋɔnɔnι wιrɛraakɛ n nιɛnɛnι.
49004030	Na-n cʋʋ haar ga-n hel Thãgbaa Thu Phuə'; ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ dɔnι jιιn Thãgba dʋ narnι dιι nιna dι taarɛ na 'lɛr dιphã waa vʋ̃ʋ, wireekɛ na ιnanι.
49004031	Nι dɔna bɩ̃ gbur fɛʋ a faa, na nĩkhii, na nĩkhi khιι, na so kιιr, na tibil i kʋɛrɛ, na bɩ̃ kpallɛsɔ fɛʋ.
49004032	Sι nι ka na bɔ khasɔ a na jɛ kha bʋɔra, a faa sopugosɔ na hana kha mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti donι nɔɔ dι Thãgba kɔɔ faarɔ anι sopugosɔ a ha nι.
49005001	Gɛr gι mɔ̃kɛ nι donι Thagbaa bιsãsɔɔkɛ a-n nanι, na-n dɔ ɔɔ phɛldara.
49005002	Na-n ιrɛ naʋra mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ na sιnι a faa ɔɔbara asι sora, a do khaardaa na bonι jir Thãgbara, kɛ hɔnι thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnaanι daʋ.
49005003	Sι ado bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ gɩ, na thɩ̃ bise cʋʋrɛ, na ha pιɛrɛ, na-n dorakɛ thιmιι ca gele n too nι nɔɔ fιιʋraka', gele na teena tιι phuusɔa';
49005004	mɛna gι dakha na yicur thιmιa, na folo folo mιιrɛ, agιbo na nɔ jι thιmιaakɛ dɔnι thιmιι bise, sι dɔ nι ka na-n mιι Thãgbaa khιι thιmιa.
49005005	Gιdonι nι jιɛ jι dι bɔdɛl cʋʋdaar, na thɩ̃ bise cʋʋdaar, na ha pιɛrdaarιkɛ mãkhananι thιl jir, na hana dιkha Kirisiti na Thãgba fãgadaarι dʋɔa'.
49005006	Na-n do tibil n gba mɔlɔ thιmιa a na-n fιιlna na', gιdonι gele n dɔ nɔɔ dι Thãgba n ιιrna nĩkhii nũ nʋʋrdarara.
49005007	Gɛr gι na-n bɔ kha fιιʋrakɛ na wele hanι thala'.
49005008	Mamara dabirə nι kɔɔ do, sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda dahɩrɛ nɩ do. Na-n hana fɩlɛɛkɛ dahɩrɛdara n hananɩ,
49005009	gɩdonɩ ka dahɩrɛ hanɩ liir bɔ cʋʋrɛ dɩɩdɩɩ, na fɩl sarʋ, na sobɔr n ha.
49005010	Nɩ mɩɛnɛ na hɩnɛ a jɛ gɩrɛ n danɩ Kɔ̃tɩn haar;
49005011	sɩ na-n bɔ kha fɩɩʋrakɛ na dabirəə thɔ̃a', gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ bʋɔ na-n the la', sɩ nɩ ka tɔ gɩ thɛna na pɛ dahɩrɛra.
49005012	Gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ tɩbɩlaale n cʋʋnι wolonena, gι-n kʋrɛrakɛ yicuru mιιrɛra.
49005013	Sι a ga thɩ̃ fɛʋʋle the dahιrɛra pι gι-n yιrrɛ mɛ̃ gbelẽ gbelẽ,
49005014	gιdonι gιrɛ dahιrɛ n caranι gι-n hιrɛrɛ. Gɛr dɔ kιrʋ dι gι so ayιwɔɔ: “Fɛrkɛ n daarɛnι, jaga, ιrɛ kherə a thɛ, Kirisiti na carã fɛr.”
49005015	Gɛr gɩ na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ anɩ ɩɩr para, na-n ɩɩr də̃bəəl khaa ga, sɩ na-n ɩrɛ dakpɛsɛ khaa.
49005016	Ƴɩɛɛkɛ nɩ yɩnɩ na-n faa gɩ ka fɩɩʋraka', gɩdonɩ bɔɔra nɛnɛ̃ waa ga bɔra'.
49005017	Gɛr gɩ na-n do jɩ 'leedara ga, sɩ na-n jɛ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ tuur.
49005018	Na-n do taan na-n kʋ na', dakhaba thɔma yɛ, sɩ nɩ ka dɔ Thu Phuu n hi ni.
49005019	Nɩ gba Thãgbaa khɩkhɩɩ nɩ, na fɔfʋɔr nɩɛ, na Thu Phuu nɩɛsɔ a na khʋɛana khasɔ. Na-n khɩna na anɩ ha fɛʋ na wireekɛ na danɩ Kɔ̃tɩn haar.
49005020	Wire fɛʋ na-n fʋɔrɛ Thãgba Thɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, gɩ do asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii irə gɩ the.
49005021	Kirisitii cʋ dɔ kɩrʋ nɩ wuro khasɔ bɩɛlbɩɛl na jɔ.
49005022	Khɛra, na-n jɔ anɩbara anɩ kora mɔ̃ nɩ-n jonɩ anɩbara Kɔ̃tɩnna.
49005023	Gɩdonɩ kuun dʋɔn yʋʋ khɛrra, mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti donɩ yʋʋ we gbɛbɩdararaakɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ tomɩ, kɛ a doronɩ gɩrɛ Taadaar.
49005024	Mɔ̃kɛ we gbɛbɩdara n jonɩ dɩbara Kirisitira, khɛra teenanɛ wɩ jɔ dɩbara ɔmɛ̃ awɩ kosɔra thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
49005025	Kona, na-n na anɩ thɛthɛɛ khɛr mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ nanɩ we gbɛbɩdara a faa ɔɔbara awɩ sora,
49005026	dɩ mɛ̃ a na lee wɩ kpɩɩ mɔ̃ a cɔcɔɔ wɩnɩ na nyʋɔn na ɔɔ thɩmɩɩ,
49005027	gɩ do nɔɔ a cʋʋ we gbɛbɩdaraalera ɓɔnanɩ wɩ jɩɩlʋʋ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, wa hana jiine na tɔtɔɔ paar dɩ dɩkhaa thɩ̃ ga, sɩ wa phure a na 'lee dɩ paar.
49005028	Mɛ̃ gɩ kona teenanɛ wa-n na awɩ thɛthɛɛ khɛr mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n nanɩ awɩ thɛthɛɛ tomɩ. Ʋrɛ naannɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ khɛr, dɩbara a na.
49005029	Gɩdonɩ tibil bɩɛl na hale n laarɛnɩ ɔɔ toma', sɩ a-n haan gɛr da-n jɩɩ tɛbɩrɩ gɩ, mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti n cʋʋnι gιrɛ we gbɛbιdara,
49005030	gιdonι sɛr dɔ ɔɔ tomι ɓã.
49005031	“Gɛr gι dι kuun na lee kha na ɔɔ thι na ɔɔ nι sι a ɓã kha na ɔɔ khɛr, wɛr yenyɔ n gbɛbι wι do tibil bιɛl”, thale gι khere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra.
49005032	Sobɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι gιιkɛ huloneni dι mɔ̃ mι yιɛnι, thale Kirisiti ha gιrɛ na ɔɔ we gbɛbιdara.
49005033	Sι ado nɛrɛ fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl gι, kuun na-n na ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ khɛr mɔ̃kɛ a-n nanι ɔɔbara, sι khɛr na-n cɔ ɔɔ ko.
49006001	Bιsana, anιda Kɔ̃tιnι ƴɛra dʋɔn, na-n nɛ anι thι na anι nι nũu, gɩdonɩ gɛr telene.
49006002	“Na cɔ afɩ thɩ na afɩ nɩ”, gɛr dɔ caca jɔfʋʋkɛ hananɩ ʋlfɛrɛ ayɩ:
49006003	“Thɩ̃ɛ na bɔ farɛ fɩ hana dakha yire fɩ pʋɔr thɩɩra.”
49006004	Sɩ nɛr thɛsɔ, na-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ gι thʋ̃ ga-n fʋ anι bιsãsɔ nĩkhiə', sι na-n haanɛ wι a na dιrɛna wι, a na naarna wι mɔ̃kɛ Kɔ̃tιn n ƴaalnι.
49006005	Dea, na-n nɛ nũu anι kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔraakɛ nι donanι kha tibil kɛ thιιra, na maar na jẽu, sι na-n cʋɛ na ha bʋɔ gι ho Kirisitira nι-n cʋʋ,
49006006	sι ga-n do awι ƴɛra dιbara gι ho tιbιla nι-n ƴaal nι da haara', sι mɔ̃kɛ nι donι Kirisitii deesɔɔkɛ n cʋɛnι gιrɛ dɔnι Thãgbaa tuur na haar fɛʋ.
49006007	Na-n dɔ war thɔma na ha bʋɔ mɔ̃ gι donι Kɔ̃tιnna nι-n do, ga do tιbιlala ga;
49006008	na-n jιnana dι tιbιla fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl, a dee ntɛ do, a waʋ ntɛ do, a na 'lɛr Kɔ̃tιnna mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ bɔ cʋʋ hanι.
49006009	Sι nɛr kɔ̃tιnasɔ, na-n cʋɛ ɔmɛ̃ na anι deesɔ; nι sɛrɔ mɔ̃ nι-n mιι warnι thιmιɩ khena, na-n jɩnana dɩ nɛrɛ na anɩ deesɔ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl nɩ hana dɩ hale ƴũ, aa-n hɩɩn tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa'.
49006010	Gɩrɛ sɛnɩ dɩphã dʋɔn wɔɔ, nɩ dɔ anɩ puno na-n the anɩ bɩɛl dora na Kɔ̃tɩn na dakha ɔɔ fãga kʋkʋra.
49006011	Nɩ gba Thãgbaa ko ke thɩ̃ fɛʋ a tɔ, a punone jɩlɛ kɩbɩ a na pɩɛrɛ Satãa fɩɩl thɔ̃ɔkɛ a-n cʋʋnɩ.
49006012	Gɩdonɩ ga do lãlaardaraakɛ dɔnɩ tɩbɩla sɩ-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna ga, sɩ fãgadara sɩ-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna, na punodara, na wɩrɛ dɔnɩ dabirə fãgadara kɛ, nakha kɔ̃tɛɛbi puusɔɔkɛ hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ.
49006013	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ nɩ gba Thãgbaa ko ke thɩ̃ fɛʋ, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ wi puu na phanɩ nɩ puno nɩ pɩɛr lãlaardaar kĩkĩ, a nɩ kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛnakɛ a dana khu paar sɩ nɩ bo nɩ jɩɩl kɩbɩ.
49006014	Gɛr gɩ nɩ fɔ gɩ ma. Nɩ gba sobɔr gɩ do lophɛrɛ nɩ khɩmɩ pelela; nɩ gba fɩl sarʋ gɩ do kũkũ kɛɛ ther;
49006015	nɩ tɔ ha ie tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩ ƴaalɛ gɩ do nɛfaa anɩ nɛra;
49006016	bɔɔ fɛʋ nɩ gba ha pɛrɛ gɩ do tomɩ phɩdaakɛ na punoneni a na khiir puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩ dɔ sõ fɛʋ;
49006017	nɩ subo dakha taarɛ gɩ do the kpɩɛr, nɩ gbana dakha Thu Phuu bajɩnaakɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa so.
49006018	Na-n bɩɛlna Thãgba na-n phʋʋrnaa anɩ bɩɛlla bɔɔ fɛʋ ga-n the Thu Phuurə; na-n jʋrɛna na yɩrrɛ, nɩ bɩɛlnɛ na pɛ tɩɩ phuusɔra fɛʋ,
49006019	na mɛrɛra dakha dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ma-n hanɩ nʋɔ ɩ̃ mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩ̃ gbullə, ɩ̃ yɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ ma gbanɩ na mɩɩna na 'lar, gɩ do gɩ yɩrrɛ casɩ.
49006020	Ga tutugo bɔɔlera mɩ doro ʋrɛ wɩ pɛrnɩ sɩ dɩ ɩ̃ bir gbãga ha gɩrɛ khaɩra; nɩ bɩɛlnɛ na pɛ mar ɩ̃ puno ma-n mɩɩ na 'lar mɔ̃kɛ gɩ teenanɩ ma-n mɩa.
49006021	Tɩsɩkɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ omineekɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ sobɔ tibil Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔna, ɔr na mɩɛnɛ nɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ hanɩ ɩ̃ pa na gɩrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n cʋʋnι.
49006022	Gɩrɛ mɩ thʋɔnaanɩ anɩ pa dʋɔn nɩ jɛ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ hanɩ asɩ pa, gɩ cʋʋ nɩ nɩ faa haar.
49006023	Ha ɩɩ, na naʋ, na ha pɛrɛ n thɛ Thãgba Thɩrɛɛ pa na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩnɩ pa a na dana omɩna fɛʋ.
49006024	Wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n naannɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na naʋʋkɛ na dɔnɩ dapɩnana', Thãgba na-n jɛ wɩ bʋɔra.
50001001	Mɛr Pol na Timothe, sɛrkɛ dɔnι Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃dara, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Jeju Kirisitii tɩɩ phusɔɔkɛ hanɩ Filipi, na we gbɛbɩdaraa hɩɩndara, na we gbɛbɩdaraa thɔ̃ dodara.
50001002	Thãgba asɩ Thɩ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn n hana nɩ ha ɩɩ a jɛ nɩ dakha bʋɔra.
50001003	Bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ ma-n jɩna nɩnɩ mɩ-n khɩɩrɛ ɩ̃ Thãgba.
50001004	Bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgba, daʋ mɩ-n bɩɛlna dɩ ma-n pɛ nar fɛʋ.
50001005	Gɩdonɩ nɩ-n bulle tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛ, dɩɩ fʋna caca wire a dana nɛnɛ̃kɛ.
50001006	Mɩ jɩrɛ tue dɩ ʋrɛ fɔnɩ anɩ hara thɔ̃ bɔ caakɛ da-n cʋʋ, a na jalna gɛr waa na ba pɩɩr Jeju Kirisitii wirə.
50001007	Gɩ teere kha ɩ̃ hana kpɩɛr caar thakɛ nɛrɛra, gɩdonɩ mɩ fʋ nɛr na ɩ̃ ha, gɩdonɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ nɩ bulle kha na mɛrɛ bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ mɩnɩ, a khaɩra mɩ ha, a ɩ̃ kɛ̃kɛrɛnaakɛ mɩ-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ n jɩlɛ kɩbɩ gɩ.
50001008	Thãgba dɔ ʋrɛ tɔ garnɩ yire dɩ ɩ̃ ha hor dɔɔ nɛrɛ fɛʋʋ sora, naʋraakɛ mɩ hana narnɩ ɓoɓo dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the.
50001009	Dɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ Thãgbara dʋɔn, anɩ naʋ n khɔna na pɩɛr wire wire na jɩɩr na kpɛsɛ hulone,
50001010	nɩ puno na-n jɩ gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ a jɔ fɛʋ, gɩ do nɔɔ nɩ phu nɩ 'lee dɩ paar Kirisitii wirə;
50001011	nɩ hinə fɩl sar beekɛ Jeju Kirisiti n cʋʋnɩ dɩ ga-n se, ga-n dʋbɩ Thãgbaa i ga-n khɩɩnaa.
50001012	Omɩna, mɩ ƴaalɛ nɩ jɛ dɩ gɩrɛ kɔɔ dana mɩnɩ ka cʋʋrɛ dɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ ka dɩ ga-n jal ƴɔɔ.
50001013	Gɩdonɩ fãgadaarɩ gardɩsɔ fɛʋ na wɩ̃ tibilsɔ paar fɛʋ jɩrɛ dɩ Kirisitiida dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ ha khaɩraakɛ.
50001014	Dɩ ɩ̃ khaɩ lona cʋʋrɛ dakha omɩna jɔɔ dɩ wɩ faa haar a ha Kɔ̃tɩn, a hanana 'lar a pɛr dɩ wa-n mɩɩna Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ, sɩ maar na-n fʋ wa'.
50001015	Sobɔr gɩ, ɩkhasɔ n mɩɩrɛ Kirisitiida na gbugi na nɔkhaa, wɛ na-n mɩɩ na ha bʋɔ kpẽgelẽ;
50001016	sɩ ha bɔdaraakɛ wer n mɩanɩ naʋra gɩ the, gɩdonɩ wɩ jɩrɛ dɩ Thãgba pɛ marɛ ɩ̃ tea na pɛ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra.
50001017	Sɩ nɔkhadaraale wer n mɩanɩ Kirisitiida, awɩ dɩbara na kpɩɛrra gɩ the, ga do bɩ̃ bʋɔra gɩ tha'. Wɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n birə na pɛ mar bɔ gaarɛ ɩ̃ khaɩdaar dora.
50001018	Anye ga cʋʋ? Gɩdonɩ a gɩ ha mɔ̃ gɩ hanɩ, gɩ dɔ bɩ̃ puu agɩbo bɩ̃ bʋɔ, sɩ Kirisitiida n mɩɩrɛ, dɩ gɩ da marɛ, sɩ ga da marɛrakɛ ga-n jalna.
50001019	Gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩrɛ tue dɩ ɩ̃ taadara gele na do fɛʋ, gι the anι Thãgba bιɛlla, na bullelaakɛ Jeju Kirisitii Thu n bulni,
50001020	mɔ̃kɛ mι-n pιɛrnι gιrɛ na haar fɛʋ, dɩ ma-n pɛna nũu, dɩ yicuru na fʋ ma', sɩ mɩ ka hananɛ 'lar a jɩ dɩ mɔ̃kɛ gɩ-n kɔɔ hanɩnakɛ wire wire mɛna ga ha nɛnɛ̃kɛ, Kirisiti na 'lɛr cʋrɛ ɩ̃ tomɩra, ado ɩ̃ yi hanana gɩ, ado ɩ̃ khirə gɩ.
50001021	Gɩdonɩ ado mɛrra gɩ, Kirisiti dɔ ɩ̃ yi hana, dɩ khir dɔ khor 'lɛdaa.
50001022	Sɩ ado ɩ̃ yi hana kɛ thɩɩra na dor nɔɔ ɩ̃ thɔ̃ na-n jal ƴɔɔ, ga dor ma jɩ gɩrɛ ma phiirni bɔɔbɔa'.
50001023	Jɛ paar yenyɔ mɩ-n jɛ: Mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ka ɩ̃ thɛ jala tɔɔ kha na Kirisiti, gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ baannɩ;
50001024	sɩ mɔ̃ ga bɔ narnɩ dɔ kɩrʋ gɩ teere kha ɩ̃ hana yire kɛ tomɩrra.
50001025	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɩ jɩnɩ tue dɩɩ do sobɔr gɩ, mɩ jɩrɛ dɩphã ma toore, ma sɩrɔrɛ sɩ ɩ̃ toona nɩ fɛʋ gɩ cʋʋ nɩ na-n bãba ha pɛrɛɛ da hanana;
50001026	dɩ mɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ ma birni wo na ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, ɩ̃dara na dor nɔɔ na-n khɩɩrɔ Jeju Kirisiti jɔɔ.
50001027	Sɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛl, nɩ hanana fɩlɛ gɩ tee kha na Kirisitii tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ ado ma pɔr na yɩ nɩ ado ma-n pɔa', sɩ ɩ̃ nɩɛ wa-n mɩɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ tɩnɩ kɩbɩ kpɩɛr bɩɛl hananɛna, dɩ na-n kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ na ha bɩɛl ha pɛ kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ tutugo bʋɔra.
50001028	Na-n do maar na-n fʋ nɩ anɩ lãlaardarasɔɔ phərəra thɩ̃ bɩɛllalaka', gɛr na nɛ war dɩ wɛr na ka na bũburõ, sɩ gɩ nɩna nɛr dɔ wɩrɛ 'lɛnɩ taarɛ dɩɩ do Thãgbara gɩ the.
50001029	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ nɛr bʋɔra, ga do dɩ na pɛ Kirisiti haar dɩbara ga, sɩ na-n gaarɛ bʋɔ ɔɔ sora.
50001030	Gɛrrara nɩ-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnɔ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ ca bɩɛlɩkɛra nɩ kɔɔ yɩ mɩnɩ dɩ ma-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna, dɩ nɩ nɩɛrɛ dɩ kɛ̃kɛrɛnɔna mɩ harakɛ gɩrɛ 'lo.
50002001	Anɩ bɩɛl do na Kirisiti dor gɩrɛ n thɔɔ nɩnɩ bɛ? Dɩ naʋ n ma narɛ bɛ? Dɩ Thu Phuu kuune n hale bɛ? Dɩ bɔ jɩ kpɩɛrɛ na bɔ fʋʋr n hale bɛ?
50002002	Nɩ cʋɛ thale daʋ n hi mar phi, mɔ̃ nɩ-n hananɩ kpɩɛr bɩɛl, na naʋ ca bɩɛl, nɩ dɔ bɩnɛ n donɩ kha bɩɛl, nɩ hanana dakha kpɩɛr ƴɛ bɩɛl.
50002003	Na-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ na dɩbara na kpɩɛrɛ na i ƴaala', sɩ nɩ dɔ dɩbara jor n cʋʋ nɩ, ʋ na-n hɩɩn ʋ, mɔ̃ a kɔ̃tɩnɩ a jʋɔ.
50002004	Na-n ƴaalɛ gɩrɛ na bɔnɩ ʋkhasɔra, ga do gɩrɛ dɔnɩ anɩda dɩbara ga.
50002005	Nɩ hanana ha caakɛ Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ hananɩ:
50002006	“Kɛkɛkɛrarakɛ bɩɛlla a do na Thãgba, sɩ aa kɔɔ hɩɩn ɔɔ Thãgba doole dɩɩ do thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a na fʋnɩ na khɩmɩnɔ kĩkĩkə̃'.
50002007	Sι ɔɔ thɛthɛ kɔɔ faa ɔɔbara sa debi a gba dee dʋʋr, a hana tomιr tibil khaa, dι mɔ̃ a debini a do tibil,
50002008	a wurre ɔɔbara a nι nũu a dana khir, kʋkʋ thιrʋra a khirakɛ ɓoɓo.
50002009	Gɛrra gɩ dɩ Thãgba thʋ̃ ɩɩrʋʋ dɩ do dakpɩɛ, a hanaa ire dɩɩ kəə iera fɛʋ.
50002010	Dɩ ireelera a hananɩ da-n do Jeju, na dor nɔɔ, nɛkhilə fɛʋ thãgbara ƴũ, na thɩɩra, a gbana tɩɛrdara fɛʋ, na gulẽgaraarɛ,
50002011	dɩ delẽbe fɛʋ na caan phasɩ nayɩ: Jeju Kirisitira dor Kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ Thãgba Thɩrɛ na 'lɛr i dʋbɩrɛ.”
50002012	Mɛ̃ gɩ ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, mɔ̃kɛ nɩ-n kɔɔ nɩ mɩnɩ nũu wire fɛʋ, na-n dɔ thɔma anɩ taarara na cʋrɛ na jẽu, ga-n do bɔɔkɛ mɩ-n hanɩ kha na nɛrɛ dɩbara ga, sɩ nɩ ka na cʋɛ ga-n jɔ mɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛ ma hanɩ kha na nɛrɛ bã.
50002013	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba dɔ ʋrɛ n pɩɛrnɩ ƴaalɛ anɩ hara na punone dɩ na-n cʋʋna gɩrɛ a-n ƴaalnɩ ga-n cʋɛ.
50002014	Na-n cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ sɩ na-n ƴɛa', na-n bana thɩ̃ banaa dakha ga;
50002015	mɛ̃ na 'lee dɩ paar, na hana sɩ paara', nɩ do Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔɔkɛ 'leanɩ sor tɩbɩlaakɛ golonenɩ a kʋɛna dakhaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, kãkɛra nɩ-n caranɩ dahɩrɛ khaa thɩɩra,
50002016	dɩ na-n 'laana yi thɩmɩɩr; thale na dɔ ɩ̃ məbida Kirisitii wi, dɩ ga do mɔlɔ mɩ kɔɔ ca ɩ̃ kɔlɔ̃kɔa', ga do mɔlɔ mɩ kɔɔ do dakha thɔma woa'.
50002017	Anɩ ha pɛ dor bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nɩ-n hanɩ Thãgba, sɩ ado gɩ teenanɛ ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃ n deere ga bonɩ jirəəle dakha, gɩ da marɛ, dɩ gɩ da marɛrakɛ wo na nɛrɛ.
50002018	Nɛrɛ dakha nɩ dɔ ga-n da nar ɔmɛ̃, dɩ nɛrɛ na mɛrɛ nɩ dɔ ga-n da sar kha.
50002019	Mɩ pɛrɛ haar ado Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn tu, kɩɛr na gbe ma thɔ̃ narɛ Timothe, ɩ̃ puno ɩ̃ nɩ anɩ tutugo ɩ̃ faa haar mer.
50002020	Gɩdonɩ ma hana tibilikɛ sɩ-n 'linəni kha ɔɔ kha, kɛ n kpɩɛrna nɩnɩ na haar vʋ̃ʋa'.
50002021	Gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ gɩrɛ na bɔ warnɩ dɩbara wɩ-n ƴaal, sɩ wa-n ka ƴaal Jeju Kirisitiida ga.
50002022	Nɩ jɩrɛ mɔ̃ jʋʋrɛ kɔɔ nɩnanɩ Timothee tιι bɔ do, dι mɔ̃kɛ bιsaan n hanι na ɔɔ thɩ, mɛ̃ a kɔɔ ha na mɛrɛ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɔna.
50002023	Mι pɛrɛ haar ɔr ma thɔ̃ dapaara ado mι jιι jɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ na ha marnɩ.
50002024	Sɩ mɩ hananɛ ha pɛrɛ gel Kɔ̃tɩnna, dɩ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na pɔr le kɩɛr na gbe.
50002025	Mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ bɔr dɩ ma thɔ̃ nar Epafʋrɔdɩtɩra ɩ̃ omi, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ sɩ kɔɔ donanɩ kha thɔma, na ʋrɛ sɩ kɔɔ kɛ̃kɛrɛnanɩ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ bɩɛl, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ nɩ kɔɔ thɔnɩ dɩ bul mi.
50002026	Gɩdonɩ anι thu fʋʋrɛ ka, dι gι pιɛraarɛ dɛr nιɛrɛraakɛ nι nιɛnι ɔɔ khora.
50002027	Sobɔr gι, gι kɔɔ khʋʋrɛ waa dɩ thɔɔ khir, sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩɩrɛ bʋɔra, sɩ ga do ɔr dɩbara Thãgbara kɔɔ jɩ bʋɔra ga, sɩ mɛrɛɛkɛrakɛ dakha, dɩ mɛ̃ ma hana gbobire na bir na dɛbɩ gbobirera ga.
50002028	Gɛr gɩ mɩ thʋɔnɛ kɔrɔ dɩ mɛ̃ ga da nar mɔ̃ na birni na yɩɩ, gɩ do nɔɔ dakha ɩ̃ gbobi n ba gbe.
50002029	Dɩ nɩ teaa na daʋ vʋ̃ʋ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ tee, na-n cɔ tibil ca wele.
50002030	Gɩdonɩ Kirisitii thɔ̃ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ danɔ khir, fɩɩʋ sɛra sɩ ɔɔ yi n bu, mɔ̃ a gbanɩ thɔmaakɛ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na kɔɔ punoni a cʋʋ mara', da-n cʋʋ.
50003001	Gɩrɛ sɛnɩ ɩ̃ omisɔ, na-n hana daʋ mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda. Ga-n yaa mɩ fɩɩʋrakɛ dɩ ma bir na 'loro gɩrɛ mɩ kɔɔ khere narnɩ mamara ga, dɩ gelela anɩ bulda gɩ do.
50003002	Na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn benasɔ, na-n jɩɛ hɩιn thɔ̃daar puusɔɔlera, na-n jιɛ hιιn wιrɛɛkɛ n ƴaalɛnι na-n liirene tomιr.
50003003	Gιdonι wιrɛ n kuroni khʋ̃ kur bʋɔ, sɛr wɛ, kɛ n fʋɔrɛnι Thãgba dιι do Thu Phuu pa gι-n the, kɛ Jeju Kirisiti donι nɔɔ dι sa-n məbi, a dona wιrɛ na-n bɔnι dι wa-n ιι gιrɛraakɛ tibil yinə n yɩna'.
50003004	Mɛrɛ dakha mι punone pɛr haar mer gιrɛraakɛ tibil yinə n yιnι, dι ado gιrɛ tibil yinə n yιnι wι yι wι bɔ na ιarɔ, ga dor mɛr ka jɔ:
50003005	Wι kɔɔ kur mer khʋ̃ʋ wire makõther wirera, Ɩjιrayɛl bire ha mι, dι ɩ̃ do Bɛ̃jamɛ̃ɛ ca, Ebirə kɔna mι dι ɩ̃ do Ebirə bʋɔ; ado jɔfʋ hιιnɛna gι, jɔfʋ bʋ dʋdaar ha mι,
50003006	ado gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃daara gι, we gbɛbιdaraa kpoodaar ha mι, ado fιl sar 'lɛrra gι jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛna, sι paar na ha mar gɛrra ga.
50003007	Sι ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera kɔɔ dɔ marnι khor, mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ mι-n hιιn gι gιrɛ dιι do, dιι do Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
50003008	Thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋrakɛ mɩ-n hιιn dιι do mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ, gι do gιrɛ baannι fĩi, kɛ dɔnι jɩɩrɩkɛ ma jɩnɩ Jeju Kirisiti ɩ̃ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ ma-n pɛr, dɔ nɔɔ; ʋrɛra dɔnɩ nɔɔ dι ɩ̃ faarɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋlera. Mι-n hɩɩn gɛr dιι do puuyʋ thιn ɩ̃ puno ɩ̃ 'lɛ Kirisiti,
50003009	ɩ̃ haaraa sι ga do na ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ fιl sarιkɛ mι 'lɛnι jɔfʋ hιιnɛna gι tha', sɩ gɩ do gɩrɛ mɩ 'lɛnɩ ha pɛrɛraakɛ mɩ hananɩ Kirisitira gɩ, kɛ dɔnι fɩl sarʋʋkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara, kɛ tibil n 'lɛnɩ ha pɛrɛra.
50003010	Mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ jɩ Kirisiti na mɔ̃ ɔɔ khi ɩɩr fãga hanɩ, ɩ̃ bul kha dakha na ɔɔ bɔ gaar, ma-n khinə khirikɛ dɔnι ɔɔda,
50003011	ma-n pɛna nũu ado ma punone a na 'lɛ khi ιιrɛ.
50003012	Ga do mι yι mι 'lɛr pa', dɩ agɩbo mɩ bɔrɛ ka pa', sɩ mɩ-n yɩrrɛ ɩ̃ 'lɛ gɩ, gɩdonɩ gɛrra Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ 'lɛ mι.
50003013	Omιna, ado mɛrra gι, ma-n kpιɛr mι 'lɛr pa'; sι thɩ̃ bιɛlιkɛ mι-n cʋʋnι dʋɔn: Mι-n diinəne gιrɛ hanι khiro, sι dι ma-n yιrna gιrɛ hanι ƴɛbʋrɔ.
50003014	Khu paar mι-n yιr ɩ̃ ca ɩ̃ dã ɩ̃ 'lɛ khorιkɛ Thãgba n we mιnι ɩ̃ 'lɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, gɩ do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
50003015	Sɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ khɔnanɩ pɩ a bɩ̃, sɩ hanana ga kpɩɛr caalera, sɩ ado anɩ kpɩɛr har kpɩɩ, Thãgba na cʋɛ gɩ dɩ ga hɩrɛ nar.
50003016	Sɩ ka sɩ danɩ gɩrɛ, sɩ fɔ ɔmɛna a ɩrɛ na jalana.
50003017	Omɩna, nɛrɛ fɛʋ nɩ dɔ ɩ̃ phɛldara, na-n hɩnɛ dakha bɔɔbɔɔ wɩrɛɛkɛ n ɩrɛnɩ mɔ̃kɛ asɩ fɩl hanɩ.
50003018	Gɩdonɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ hale awɩ ɩɩr para wɩ dor Kirisitii kʋkʋ thɩr lãlaardara; mɩ-n kɔɔ mɩɛ nɛr bɔɔ jɔɔjɔɔ awɩda, na nɛnɛ̃kɛrakɛ mɩ-n mɩɩ gɛr 'lo na bɩwɛ dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ:
50003019	Awɩ khu pa na dor bũburone, gɩrɛ n danɩ awɩ tomɩra dɔrɔɔm dʋɔn awɩ thãgba, awɩ yicur cʋʋ wι-n khιι, wa-n kpιɛrna thɩ̃ɛ saagado thɩɩkɛɛ thɩ̃ gaaga.
50003020	Sɩ se wer, asɩ dɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ ha, le Taadaarɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιnɩkɛ sɩ-n pɩɛrnɩ na the na ɩ̃.
50003021	Ɔr na deba asɩ tomɩɩkɛ yɔɔnɩ a cʋʋ gɩ hona ɔɔ tomɩɩkɛ ɓɔnanɩ, gɩ the ɔɔ fãgaraakɛ a hananɩ a cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ gɩ jʋʋraa.
50004001	Mɛ̃ gɩ, ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, kɛ n kɔ mɩnɩ thue, nɛrkɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ kãkada na ɩ̃ məbida, nɩ tɛ kɩbɩ gɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra, nɛrkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ.
50004002	Mɩ-n bɩɛlɛ Evodɩ, mɩ-n bɩɛlɛ Sɛ̃tɩsɩ dɩ wa 'li kha mɔ̃ wɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda.
50004003	Dɩ fɛrɛ dakha, kɛ dɔnɩ yʋ gbuu tibil thɔmana, mɩ-n bɩɛl fɛr dɩ fa bul wi, gɩdonɩ wɛr kɔɔ tɛrɔ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛ nakha mɛrɛ, na Kilemã na wɩ̃ tibil ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ dɔna mɩnɩ kha thɔma, kɛ awɩ i hanɩ yi sɛbɛra.
50004004	Na-n hana daʋ wire fɛʋ mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda, ɔɔ mɩ bire so wo na-n hana daʋ.
50004005	Dɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na-n yɩ mɔ̃ nɩ hananɩ hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ. Kɔ̃tɩn wɔrɔnɛ dɔdɔdɔ.
50004006	Na-n jẽ haar thɩ̃ bɩɛllalaka', sɩ thɩɛna fɛʋ na-n sɔ Thãgbara gɩrɛ n ɓɔra nɩnɩ na bɩɛlɛ, na phʋʋrɛ, na fʋɔrɛ.
50004007	Dɩ Thãgbaa ha ieekɛ kəəneni dɩ tibil na-n jɩ kɩrʋa', na-n bɛra anɩ ha na anɩ kpɩɛr mɔ̃ nɩ hanɩ Jeju Kirisitira.
50004008	Gɩrɛ sɛnɩ omɩna, nɩ dɔ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnι sobɔr, na gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ teananι cʋʋr, na gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ telenenι, na gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ phonɩ, na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ danananɛ, na gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ thɛnɩ ire, na thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ thʋnanɩ ɓɔ̃ ka a teena khɩirɛ, n do anɩ kpɩɛrnɔ.
50004009	Gɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ, kɛ nɩ 'lɛnɩ ɩ̃ pa, na gɩrɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ a yɩna gɩ ɩ̃ pa, na-n cʋɛ gɛr, dɩ Thãgbaakɛ ha ɩɩ n thernɩ na ha kha na nɛrɛ.
50004010	Mɩ-n khɩɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn na daʋ ka gɩrɛraakɛ nɩ birni a kpɩɛrna mɩ wo. Nɩ kɔɔ mãa kpɩɛrna gar wer, sɩɩ do fʋ paar ɓɔra nɩ.
50004011	Ga do ɩ̃ thɩ̃ ɓɔra dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma-n mɩɩ thaka', gɩdonɩ a mɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ mɩ hanɩnakɛ, sɩ gɩ-n da marɛ.
50004012	Mɩ-n marrɛ dɩ ɩ̃ too na thɩ̃ 'leere, mɩ-n marrɛ dɩ ɩ̃ too ado mɩ hana thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ; thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra na paar fɛʋ, mɩ jɩrɛ thɩ̃ doo n dɔnɩ hiir na thɩ̃ doo n dɔnɩ kɔmɛr, a jɩ thɩ̃ jɔ hananɛ na thɩ̃ ɓɔrɛ.
50004013	Mɩ-n punone thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ cʋʋ dɩ gɩ the fãgaraakɛ Kirisiti n pɛ marnɩ;
50004014	sɩ gɩ bɔrɛrakɛ nɩ kɔɔ bul mini ɩ̃ bɔ gaarra.
50004015	Nɛr Filipidara nɩ jɩrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ma kɔɔ thenɩ Masedʋan caca bɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ, nɛr dɔ we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ dɩbara kɔɔ bulo mini na war thɩmɩɩr.
50004016	Gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ hanɩ Tesalonɩkɩ, nɩ kɔɔ thɔnanɛ khaardaa balanyɔsɔ a ha mɩ dɩɩ bul mi ɩ̃ thɩ̃ ɓɔrra.
50004017	Ga do khaardaa mɩ-n ƴaala', sɩ gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ dʋɔn khorɩkɛ gelela n ɩna narnɩ.
50004018	Mɩ 'lɛr thɩɛna fɛʋ dɩ thɩ̃ jɔdaar ha mɩ, nyɔ̃korʋ hi mer phi na khaardaakɛ Epafʋrɔdɩtɩ kɔɔ thenanɩ anɩ pa a ɩna ha mɩ; thɩ̃ɛ gɩɩkɛ n hʋnanɩ Thãgba daʋ latɩkolo khaa, a dʋʋraa bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ daaraanɩ haar dɩ tee.
50004019	Ɩ̃ Thãgba na ha nɛr thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n ɓɔra nɩnɩ, mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ leekɛ a lenɩ dɩɩ və̃vĩə hanɩ, gɩ do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
50004020	Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Thɩ ɔɔ i n dʋbarɔ na jala waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ.
50004021	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl, kɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii too. Omɩnaakɛ hanɩ kha na mɛrɛ wɩ fʋɔr nɛr.
50004022	Tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋ fʋɔr nɛr, sɩ cacara Sejaarɩ cɔdara wɛ.
50004023	Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn na-n jɛ nɩ fɛʋ bʋɔra.
51001001	Mɛr Polιkɛ dɔnι Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni na Timothe asι omi,
51001002	thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha tιι phuusɔɔkɛ dɔnι sobɔ omιna, kɛ Kirisiti hιnι dι wι ha Kolosι. Thãgba asι Thι n hana nι ha ιι a jɛ nι dakha bʋɔra.
51001003	Wire koo sι-n khιι Thãgba asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii Thι dι sι bιɛlnaa dι sa-n pɛ nar,
51001004	gιdonι sι nιɛrɛ mɔ̃ nι pɛnι Jeju Kirisiti haar na naʋʋkɛ nι hananι tιι phuusɔra fɛʋ.
51001005	Gιdonι ɔbɔɔkɛ sobɔ thιmιιrιkɛ dɔnι tutugo bʋɔ kɔɔ danι anι pa gι cʋʋ nɛr dɩ nɩ jɩ nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ gɩ-n 'laanɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ anɩ ha pɛ na anɩ naʋ jɩɩl gɩrɛraakɛra nɩ-n pɛnɩ nũu, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba thɩɩn narnɩ le ƴũ.
51001006	Dɩ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛra ƴɛrrɛ a pɩ paar fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ, a ha mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ danɩ anɩ pa dabɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ cacara Thãgbaa bɔ jɩda, dɩ nɩ kɔɔ jɩ gɛr dɩɩ do gɛr dɔ sobɔr.
51001007	Epafɩrasɩɩkɛ sɩ-n nanɩ, kɛ sɩ donanɩ kha thɔ̃ dona ɔr kɔɔ dɩrɛ nɩ, sobɔ tibil gɩ Kirisitii thɔna anɩ sora;
51001008	ɔr mɩɛnɛ sɩ naʋ caakɛ Thu Phuu kɔɔ pɛ narnɩ.
51001009	Gɛr gɩ dɩ sɛrɛ dakha a fʋna wireekɛ sɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ, sa-n pɩr kpɩɩ sa-n bɩɛl Thãgba sa-n pɛ naraa ga. Sɩ-n bɩɛlɛ dɩ na 'lɛ kpɛsɛrɛ na jɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thu Phuuda, a na jɩna gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa tuur bɔɔbɔɔ.
51001010	Mɛ̃ na hana fɩlɛ na-n ɩɩr mɔ̃ Kɔ̃tɩn n ƴaalnɩ na-n cʋʋ gɩrɛ n daaraanɩ haar wire fɛʋ, na-n cʋʋna thɔ̃ bɔ caar dɩɩdɩɩ, anɩ Thãgba jɩ n kɔ̃tɩ̃ dakha ga-n pɛr.
51001011	Ɔɔ fãgaakɛ na hanɩ mɩɛrɛra ga n cʋɛ nɩ nɩ 'lɛ punone thɩɛna fɛʋ dɩɩdɩɩ, gɩ do nɔɔ na-n yɩr na ha fʋrɛ na daʋ.
51001012	Na-n fʋɔrɛ Thɩrɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ hana nɩnɩ punone dɩ na 'lɛ anɩda na tɩɩ phuusɔ ɔɔ fãga dɩ hɩrɛra.
51001013	Ɔr kɔɔ taa sɩ dabirəə fãgara, sa gba sɩ a pɛ ɔɔ Bikuunikɛ a nanɩɩ fãga dɩra.
51001014	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ birsene sini a faa asɩ sopugosɔ a ha sɩ.
51001015	Kirisitiikɛ dɔnɩ dayɩnanɛ ɔr n nɛ sar mɔ̃ Thãgbaakɛ na dɔnɩ dayɩnana' hanɩ. Ɔr dɔ cacadaarɩkɛ Thãgba kɔnɩ dɩ do yʋʋ thɩ̃ tinənena fɛʋ;
51001016	gɩdonɩ ɔɔ pa thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ tenɩ the, gɩrɛ hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ na thɩɩra, kɛ dɔnɩ dayɩnanɛ na gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ dayɩnana', a thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ dakpɛna yʋʋsɔ wɛ, na kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, na fãgadarasɔ, na punodarasɔ. Ɔr Thãgba tinə thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ ɔɔ ti gɩ ti.
51001017	Ɔr kɔɔ haanle sɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ ti pa'; ɔr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ ha dapa a too.
51001018	Ɔr dɔ yʋʋ tomιrraakɛ dɔnι we gbɛbιdara; ɔr dɔ caca fʋ paar, cacadaarɩkɛ Thãgba kɔnɩ gɩ, kɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ a the khirera, gɩ dɔ nɔɔ ɔr n do cacadaar thɩɛna fɛʋ.
51001019	Gɩdonɩ gɩ dar Thãgba haar dι mɔ̃kɛra a hanɩ ɔmɛna ɔɔ Bikuun na ha gbelẽ gbelẽ.
51001020	Gɩ daaraarɛ dakha haar dɩ gba ɔɔ Bikuun a cʋʋna thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩ gɩ bir kũu kha na ɔr Thãgba, ado gɩrɛ hanɩ thɩɩra gɩ, ado gɩrɛ hanɩ thãgbara ƴũ gɩ; ɔɔ Bikuuni tɔmɩ̃ɩkɛ kɔɔ deerenɩ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra dɔ nɔɔ dɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ bir 'lɛrɔ ha ɩɩ na Thãgba.
51001021	Nɛrɛ dakha mamara nɩ kɔɔ dor kpakpala Thãgbaadara na ɔɔ lãlaardara, dɩɩ the anɩ kpɩɛrra na anɩ puu cʋʋra.
51001022	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ Thãgba cʋʋ nɛr dɩ nɩ bir kũu kha na ɔr, dɩι the ɔɔ Bikuuni khirə mɔ̃ a debini a do tibil, gι cʋʋ nι nι jιιl ɔɔ ƴɛ thɩ̃thιιn nι phu, nι 'lee dι paar, na hana sι paara';
51001023	ado nι fʋrɔrɛ ha pɛrɛ dι na-n jalna a jιιllɔ a ma kĩkĩ, dι ga do nι kɛrrɛ sa faa nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ nι hananι dιι the tutugo bʋɔraakɛ nι kɔɔ nιɛna', kɛ dɔnι gιrɛ wι kɔɔ mιιnι tιbιlala fɛʋ thιιra, kɛ mɛr Pol doronι gιrɛ thɔ̃ don.
51001024	Nɛnɛ̃ daʋ fʋ mɛr ka ɩ̃ bɔ gaarraakɛ mι-n gaarnι nɛrɛra; bʋɔɔkɛra mι-n gaarnι ɩ̃ tomιra, Kirisitii we gbɛbιdaraa sora, kɛ dɔnι ɔɔ tomι, gι ɓaanɛ dι ga-n pιιr Kirisitiidaakɛ a kɔɔ gaarnι awι sora;
51001025	dι we gbɛbιdaraa thɔ̃ dodaarra mι do gιrɛ, dιι ha mɔ̃ thɔmaakɛ Thãgba pɛ marnι ma-n dɔ nar hanι, gɛr dʋɔn ma-n mιa ɔɔ thιmιι koo,
51001026	kɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ gbulikɛ kɔɔ keranι kɛkɛkɛ tιbιlala fɛʋ, sι Thãgba cʋʋ gι dι gι yιr nɛnɛ̃ ɔɔ tιι phusɔra.
51001027	Thãgbaa ƴaalla gι the dι cʋʋ wι wι jɛ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ gbullə donι thɩ̃ ɓʋ̃ɔ ka a kpaa nʋɔ tibil caarra fɛʋ, gɛr dʋɔn: Kirisiti ha anι bιnɔ, kɛ dɔnι nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ nι hananι mɔ̃ na 'lɛnι i dʋbιrɛ na Thãgba.
51001028	Ɔr dɔ Kirisitira sι-n mιιnι. Sι-n kpãkpaanɛ tιbιlala fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl dι sa-n dιιrna wι na kpɛsɛrɛ fɛʋ, gι cʋʋ tιbιla fɛʋ wι bɔr wι ka Thãgbaa ƴɛra, gι the awι bιɛl dora na Kirisiti.
51001029	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dι ma-n gbũgbulõ thɔmana dι ma-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna gι, na Kirisitii fãga kʋkʋʋkɛ a ha mιnι dι ga-n do thɔma ɩ̃ pa.
51002001	Gιdonι mι-n ƴaalɛ nι jɛ mɔ̃ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ιkɛ mι-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnι anι sora hanι, na wιrɛraakɛ hanι Laʋdιse, na wιrɛraakɛ na yɛ mιnι ƴɛbiro pa',
51002002	gι do nɔɔ wɩ yɩ ha ƴɔllɛ, wɩ gbɛbɩ wɩ do bɩɛl naʋra, wι hana tu jιιrιkɛ thɛnι jι bʋɔra, wι puno wa-n jιna Thãgbaa thɩ̃ gbulikɛ dɔnι Kirisitii thɛthɛ.
51002003	Ɔr cʋɛ Thãgbaa kpɛsɛ na jιιrιkɛ hɔnι tιι ko thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ keranι dιι yιr.
51002004	Mι-n mιιrɛ thakɛ gι do nɔɔ tibil na fιιl nι na nɔ da thιmιa ga.
51002005	Mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na hanɩ anɩ parakɛ gɩra', sɩ ɩ̃ thu har kha na nɛrɛ, dɩ daʋ fʋ mɛr mɔ̃ mɩ yɩnɩ fɩl bʋɔ dɩɩ ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, na mɔ̃ anɩ ha pɛɛkɛ nɩ hananɩ Kirisitira tɩnɩ kĩkĩ.
51002006	Mɛ̃ gɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ 'lɛnɩ Jeju Kirisiti dɩ do Kɔ̃tɩn, na-n ɩrɛ kha na ɔr na wa fɩl,
51002007	a gɔ nɛɛ gɩ hulono ɔrra; nɩ jɩlɛ ɔrra kɩbɩ, nɩ tɛ ha pɛrɛraakɛ nɩ hananɩ mɔ̃kɛ dɩɩrɛɛkɛ wɩ kɔɔ dɩɩr nɩnɩ hanɩ. Nɩ dɔ Thãgba khɩɩrɛ n too nɩ nɔɔ.
51002008	Na-n jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, na-n do tibil n fʋ nɩ a ɩɩrɔ na tibil jɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ mɔlɔdaa wɩ-n fɩɩlna nɩna', gele fɛʋ kpamna gɩ the na dɩɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ bɔ taa dɩɩra', kɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ tinəneeda, ga do Kirisitii pa gɩ tha'.
51002009	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba dʋʋr koo har Kirisitii tomɩra.
51002010	Dɩ anɩ yi hanana na Kirisiti, dɩkha na ɓɔr nɩ fɩɩʋraka'. Ɔr dɔ yʋʋ kɔ̃tɩnasɔra fɛʋ na fãgadarasɔra fɛʋ.
51002011	Mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ kha bɩɛl na Kirisiti wɩ kɔɔ kur nar khʋ̃ʋ, sɩ ga do tibil nyɛ̃ɛ kuro ga, sɩ Kirisiti n kuro gɩ; a thɩɛna gaa gɛr dɔ taarɛ tɩɩ tɩ̃ dʋʋrra.
51002012	Yɔ kpɛɛrɛra wɩ kɔɔ dʋ nɩ kha na Kirisiti, sɩ Thãgba ɩɩr nɩ kha dakha khirera wo na ɔrra, dɩɩ the ha pɛrɛraakɛ nɩ hananɩ Thãgbaa fãgaraakɛ kɔɔ cʋgɛɛnɩ dɩ ɩɩr a the khirera.
51002013	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mamara anɩ sopugo na mɔ̃ na kɔɔ kurni khʋ̃a' dɔnɩ nɔɔ dɩ nɩ kɔɔ khi, sɩ nɛnɛ̃ Thãgba bire ha nɩ kha yire na Kirisiti a faana asɩ sopugosɔ fɛʋ.
51002014	Jɔfʋʋkɛ kɔɔ kheranɩ asɩ so heen khere dɩɩ do a thɩɛna gaa sor heene sɩ asɩ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ kʋɛrara, Thãgba bũburõ ger a faa mɔ̃ a gba gɩnɩ a kpa thɩrʋra.
51002015	Kʋkʋ thιrʋʋ pa gι the dι Kirisiti puno kɔ̃tιnasɔ na fãgadarasɔɔ fãga a tagιrι, sa nιna tιbιla fɛʋ dι ɔr punone wi.
51002016	Gɛr gι na-n do tibil n yι hʋɛ a na-n yι nar dιι gιrɛraakɛ nι-n khonι dι na-n yɔna ga, agιbo gι do fɛtι thιmιιrra, na sιpo pha hιιndaara dι hιιr widaara gι woa'.
51002017	Gelesɔ fɛʋ dʋɔn gιrɛ na ɩnanɩɩ jəər, sι gιrɛ dɔnι sobɔ bire Kirisiti gι.
51002018	Na-n do tibil n fιιl nι na sõso dιbara jor, na thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔ fʋɔrda, gι cʋʋ nι nι 'lee khorιkɛ na 'lɛna'. Tibil ca ole ire a-n ka thιɛnaakɛ a yιnι ιnι yɩrɛ, gɩdonι ɔɔ kpɩɛrra aa-n kpιɛrna Thãgba ga;
51002019	sι aa-n ka dι ma Kirisitiraakɛ dɔnɩ yʋa', kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ n cʋɛnɩ tomɩr fɛʋ dɩ ɔɔ ƴɔɔ pa na cela fɛʋ n li gi dɩɩ coor a do bɩɛl, a khɔ̃ dɩɩ do Thãgbaa pa gɩ the.
51002020	Gɩdonɩ nɩ kɔɔ khire kha na Kirisiti, na ha kha dιkha na dιιrɛɛkɛ na dɔnι bɔ taa dιιra', kɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ tinəneeda ga, mɔ̃gιdo dι na hana fιlɛ 'lo gι ho thιιkɛɛda nι do, nι sιrɔ wa-n ha nι jɔfʋ wι yι:
51002021	Fa-n gba ga, fa-n 'lɛ hιιna', fa-n thara'.
51002022	Sι gelesɔ fɛʋ thɩ̃ kʋɛna gι do a fι yι fι gba gι a na cʋɛna thɩ̃ɛ, dιrakɛ wo tibil jɔfʋ gι na tibil dιιrɛ.
51002023	A fι yιɛ wer gι-n hʋrɛ kpɛsɛrɛ, mɔ̃ gι-n hananι dιbara fɛrɛ Thãgba fʋɔrɛ, na dιbara jor, na tomι hʋɔlɛ dιbara, sιι dorakɛ ga do bɔ taa thɩ̃ɛ ha gela', sι tomιrιkɛ gι-n kʋnɩ thue dɔrɔɔm, dɩɩ do gɩ daaraarɛ gɩ.
51003001	Mɔ̃ nɩ ɩɩrnɩ khirera nakha Kirisiti, na-n ƴaalɛ ƴũ thɩ̃ɛ, ka Kirisiti hanɩ gɩrɛ a too Thãgbaa nyɔ̃bɔra.
51003002	Na-n kpɩɛrna ƴũ thɩ̃ɛ, na-n kpɩɛrna gɩrɛ hanɩ thɩɩra ga.
51003003	Gɩdonɩ nɩ kɔɔ khire dɩ anɩ yi ha Kirisitira dɩphã a ker Thãgbaa pa.
51003004	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Kirisitiikɛ dɔnɩ anɩ yi hana na yɩrnɩ, le na yɩr kha dakha na ɔr ɔɔ i dʋbɩra.
51003005	Gɛr gɩ nɩ kɔ anɩ thɩ thɩ̃ ƴaal, kɛ dɔnɩ bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ, na thɩ̃ bise cʋʋrɛ, na thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛ, na thɩ̃ puu kpɩɛrɛ, na ha pɩɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ bɩɛl na thɩl jir.
51003006	Gɛrra n cʋɛ nĩkhii dɩɩ fʋ Thãgba.
51003007	Dɩ nɛrɛ dakha nɩ kɔɔ hananɛ ga fɩlɩlera mamara ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ kɔɔ ha garnɩ.
51003008	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ nɩ dɔna gelesɔ fɛʋ a faa: Nĩkhii, nĩkhi khɩɩ, kpallɛ, tibil i kʋɛrɛ na khaakhaar thɩmɩaakɛ n thɛnɩ anɩ nɔra.
51003009	Na-n kuur sɔ̃sɔ na pɛ khasɔa', gɩdonɩ nɩ kɔɔ thʋbɩrɛ tɩɩ tɩ̃ dʋʋr na ɔɔ thɔ̃ a faa,
51003010	sa to tɩɩ pha dʋʋrɩkɛ n dʋɔnnɩ daphaa da-n pɛr, da-n hona Thãgbaakɛ tieni dɩ a na jɩɩ hananaa jɩ bʋɔ.
51003011	Liir Juifi na ha kpɩɩ dɩ wɩrɛ na dɔnɩ Juifisɔa ha kpɩa', dɩ ʋrɛ wɩ kurni khʋ̃ʋ gɩ dɩ ʋrɛ wa kurni khʋ̃aa ga, dɩ hɔ̃ baldara wɛ dɩ wɩrɛ na phuoni yire paa ga, dɩ dee gɩ dɩ waʋ ga; sɩ Kirisiti dʋɔn thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ a har dakha thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
51003012	Gɛr gɩ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ donɩ wɩrɛ Thãgba phiirni dɩ nɩ phu, a dona dakha wɩrɛ a-n nanɩ, nɩ hanana bɔ jɩɩr gɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ gɩ ka, na ha bulo fɩlɛ, na dɩbara jor, na hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ, na ha fʋrɛ.
51003013	Ado tibil hana sor na ʋ̃ tibil, nɩ hanana kha ha fʋrɛ a faa na hana kha; mɔ̃kɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ faanι anι sopugosɔ, nɛrɛ dakha nι faa sopugosɔ na hana kha.
51003014	Sι gιrɛ jɔnιnakɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dʋɔn nι hanana naʋʋkɛ dʋɔnnι bιɛl do lidaakɛ n cʋɛnι tibil dι bɔr dι ka.
51003015	Ha ιιkɛ n thɛnι Kirisitira, kɛ Thãgba we narnι nι 'lɛ mɔ̃ nι donι tomι bιɛl, nι dɔ ha ιιra n do kɔ̃tιn anι hara, na-n hana dakha fɔfʋɔr haar.
51003016	Nι dɔ Kirisitii thιmιιkɛ ɓɔnanι ka n too anι hara jɔɔ. Na-n dιrɛ kha thɩ̃ɛ a na kpãkpaana khasɔ bιɛlbιɛl na kpɛsɛrɛ fɛʋ. Na-n khιna Thãgbaa khιkhιι nι, na ɔɔ fɔfʋɔr nι, na Thu Phuu nιɛsɔ; na-n khιna gιsɔ na fɔfʋɔr haar ga-n khιι Thãgba.
51003017	Dι thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nι-n cʋʋnɩ, a thɩmɩɩr nɩ-n mɩɩ, a thɔma nɩ-n do, na-n cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩda, a na khɩana Thãgba Thɩrɛ gɩ do ɔɔda dɔ nɔɔ.
51003018	Khɛra, na-n jɔ anɩbara anɩ kora mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda.
51003019	Kona, na-n na anɩ khɛr, na-n hananaa fɩl khɩa'.
51003020	Bɩsana, na-n nɛ anɩ thɩ na anɩ nɩ nũu thɩɛna fɛʋ, gɩdonɩ gɛr n da Kɔ̃tɩn haar.
51003021	Thɛ, na-n gba bɩsanana fɩl khɩɩ awɩ kpɩɛr n kʋɛa'.
51003022	Dea, na-n nɛ nũu thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra anɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔraakɛ nɩ donanɩ kha tibil kɛ thɩɩra, sɩ ga-n do awɩ ƴɛra dɩbara gɩ ho tɩbɩla nɩ-n ƴaal nɩ da haara', sɩ na-n cʋɛ na ha bʋɔ gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩn nɩ-n ma.
51003023	Thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ nɩ-n cʋʋnɩ na-n cʋɛ na haar fɛʋ, gɩ ho Kɔ̃tɩnna nɩ-n cʋʋ ga-n do tɩbɩlala ga;
51003024	na-n jɩnana dɩ Kɔ̃tɩn na ka nɩ na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a thɩɩnnɩ gɩ dɔ anɩda. Gɩdonɩ Kirisiti dʋɔn Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ nɩ-n doronɩ thɔma.
51003025	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛnɩ puure a na 'lɛr lɩmɩnɛ ɔɔ puu cʋʋrara, dɩɩdɩɩ hɩɩnɛ na hala'.
51004001	Kɔ̃tɩna, nɩ telene a bʋɔnɔ anɩ deesɔra, na-n jɛna dɩ nɛrɛ dakha nɩ hananɛ bɩɛl dɩ do Kɔ̃tɩn a ha ƴũ.
51004002	Na-n yɩra Thãgba bɩɛlɛla, nɩ hanana gar pərre a na khɩa Thãgba.
51004003	Nɩ jɩɛ bɩɛlna dakha Thãgba na pɛ sar, Thãgba n khɛr sɩ loo Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ Kirisitii thɩmɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ gbul, kɛ dɔnɩ nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ ha gɩrɛ khaɩra,
51004004	ɩ̃ puno ma-n jɩɩ mɩɩ gɩ gɩ yɩr casɩ mɔ̃kɛ gɩ teenanɩ.
51004005	Na-n hana kpɛsɛrɛ wɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ ha pɛdara ga. Ƴɩɛɛkɛ nɩ yɩnɩ na-n faa gɩ ka fɩɩʋraka'.
51004006	Wire fɛʋ nɩ dɔ anɩ thɩmɩɩ na-n do gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ, gɩ dɔ thɩmɩɩ daa, nɩ jɩ mɔ̃ na birseni tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
51004007	Tɩsɩkɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ omineekɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ sobɔ tibilikɛ sɩ donanɩ kha thɔ̃ dona Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔna, ɔr na mɩɛnɛ nɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ hanɩ ɩ̃ pa.
51004008	Gɩrɛ mɩ thʋɔnaanɩ anɩ pa dʋɔn nɩ jɛ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ hanɩ asɩ pa, gɩ cʋʋ nι nι faa haar.
51004009	Mι thʋɔnɛ nakha Onejιmιkɛ dɔnι sobɔ tibil, a dona omineekɛ mι-n nanι, kɛ dɔnι dakha anι tibil. Wɛr na mιɛnɛ nι mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ hanι kɛkɛ.
51004010	Arιsιtarkιιkɛ sι hananι kha khaιra a fʋɔr nɛr, na dakha Markιιkɛ dɔnι Barnabasιι omi, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛɛkɛ mι kɔɔ so narnι ayι: Ado a pɔ anι pa nι teaa.
51004011	Jejuukɛ wι-n wenι Jusitusi a fʋɔr nɛr dakha. Khʋ̃ kurdaraa thɩ̃thιιn, wɛr yẽther dιbara dɔ tιbιlaakɛ n dɔna mιnι kha Thãgbaa fãgadaar do thɔma; wɛr dɔ wιrɛ n kɔɔ ƴɔla mιnι haar.
51004012	Epafιrasιιkɛ dɔnι anι tibil a fʋɔr nɛr; Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃daar a do; bɔɔ fɛʋ a-n kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ Thãgba bιɛlɛla da-n pɛ nar, gι dɔ nɔɔ nι jιιl kιbι mɔ̃ nι donι ha pɛdaraakɛ bιnanι, a hana tu jιιr dɩ na-n cʋʋ gιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba tuni.
51004013	Mι punone so ɔɔdara ayι: Tibil gιιkɛ n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛnι thɔmana anι sora, na wιrɛraakɛ hanɩ Laʋdɩse na Yerapolɩsɩ.
51004014	Luki dɔtɔrɔ kuunikɛ sɩ-n nanɩ na dakha Demasɩ n fʋɔr nɛr.
51004015	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ omɩnaakɛ hanɩ Laʋdɩse na Nɛ̃fasɩ na we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ n gbɛbanɩ kha ɔɔ cɔ.
51004016	Ado sɛbɛɛkɛ hɩɩn anɩ pa pɩ, nɩ dɔ dakha wɩ hɩɩn gɩ Laʋdιse we gbɛbιdarara, nɛrɛ dakha n hιιn ʋrɛ na thɛnι Laʋdιsedaraa pa.
51004017	Sι nι sɔ Arsιpιra ayɛwɔɔ, a na-n jιɛ hιιn thɔmaakɛ a kɔɔ 'lɛnι Kɔ̃tιnι pa, a cʋɛ gι ga-n dã bɔɔbɔɔ.
51004018	Mɛr Polι thɛthɛ khera fʋɔrɛɛkɛ na ɩ̃ nyɛ̃. Na-n jɛna mɔ̃ mι hanι khaιra. Thãgba na-n jιɛ nι bʋɔra.
52001001	Mɛr Pol na Sιlvɛ̃ na Timothe thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha we gbɛbιdaraakɛ hanι Tesalonιkι, kɛ Thãgba Thιrɛ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιn hιnι. Thãgba n hana nι ha ιι a jɛ nι dakha bʋɔra.
52001002	Wire fɛʋ sι-n khιι Thãgba nɛrɛ fɛʋʋdara, dι sι bιɛlna Thãgba dι sa-n pɛ nar na anι i.
52001003	Bɔɔ fɛʋ sɩ-n jɩna asɩ Thɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, anɩ ha pɛ thɩ̃ cʋʋ, na anɩ naʋ thɔ̃ cʋʋ, na anɩ kɩbɩ jɩɩl, nũ pɛrɛraakɛ nɩ hananɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira.
52001004	Sɩ jɩrɛ tue omɩna dɩ Thãgba naan nɩ a kɔɔ phiir ni.
52001005	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩkɛ sɩ kɔɔ pɔnanɩ, ga do nʋɔ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩna dɩbara ga, sɩ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ gɛr dɩɩ ha phãphãphã, na Thu Phuu, na tu jɩɩr vʋ̃ʋ; gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ fɩl caakɛ sɩ kɔɔ hananɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn gɩ do nɔɔ thɩ̃ɛ n bɔ nar.
52001006	Dɩ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛrakɛ debire a do asɩ ph ɛldara na Kɔ̃tɩnɩ phɛldara kpoore jɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn, kɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩraakɛ nɩ-n 'lɛnɩ na daʋʋkɛ n thɛnɩ Thu Phuurə,
52001007	a thʋ̃ debi waa a do thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ ha pɛdarara fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ Masedʋan na Akaɩ.
52001008	Sɩ ga do Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩ kɔɔ ther anɩ pa dɩ ga-n kpaar dɩ Masedʋandara na Akaɩdara nɩɛ dɩbara ga, sɩ paar fɛʋ wɩ nɩrɛ mɔ̃ anɩ ha pɛ Thãgbara hanɩ, dɩ ga do gɩ thʋnɛ harakɛ mɩɩrɛra dɩ sa mɩɩ bã.
52001009	Gɩdonɩ wɩ-n mɩɩrɛ asɩda teereraakɛ nɩ kɔɔ tee sɩnɩ ɓoɓo, na dakha wo mɔ̃kɛ nɩ kɔɔ kɛrnɩ a pɛr Thãgba haar sa faa thɩla, sɩ nɩ do thɔma Thãgba yidaarraakɛ dɔnɩ Thãgba bɔ,
52001010	na-n pɩɛrna dakha ɔɔ Bikuunikɛ na thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, kɛ dɔnɩ Jejuukɛ a kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ dɩ the khirera, kɛ dɔnɩ asɩ tataa Thãgbaa nĩkhirəəkɛ n ɩnanɩ.
52002001	Omɩna, nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ jɩrɛ dɩ asɩ pɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ pɔnɩ anɩ pa na kɔɔ do mɔlɔa'.
52002002	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ gaarnɩ bʋɔ a 'lɛna kpoore jɔɔ Filipira pɩ, mɔ̃kɛ nɩ jɩ gɩnɩ dɩɩ kɔɔ ha, sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ ha sɛr 'lar mɔ̃kɛ sɩ pɔnɩ dɩ sa-n mɩɩ nɩ Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ bãbaranɛ jɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn.
52002003	Asɩ wewe Thãgba thɩmɩɩkɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ na kɔɔ the dədirrə dɩ kpɩɛr puurə ga, dɩ ga kɔɔ do dakha fɩɩl thɩmɩa ga.
52002004	Gɩ ka har mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ jʋʋr sɩnɩ hɩɩn dɩ sɩ teena dɩ heen sɩ tutugo bʋɔɔle, mɛ̃ sɩ-n mɩɩ gɩ, ga do dɩ sa da tɩbɩla haara', sɩ dɩ sa da Thãgba haar, kɛ n bəəreni asɩ bɩ̃ dɩ jɩ mɔ̃kɛ gɩ hanɩ.
52002005	Nι jιrɛ mɔ̃kɛ gι kɔɔ hanι, ga do fιιl thιmιιr sι kɔɔ mιι nι kpιιraka', dι sa kɔɔ phɩ̃ nar dakha fιlɛ thʋnɔ, sι sa-n ƴaal nar dιkha ga, Thãgbaa thɛthɛ torre yire;
52002006	dι dakha sa kɔɔ ƴaal i dʋbιrɛɛkɛ thɛnι tιbιlaa pa, dι anι pa gι, dι ʋkhasɔɔ pa ga.
52002007	Mɔ̃kɛ sι donιnakɛ Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔna, sι kɔɔ punone a na nιna asι kɔ̃tɩ̃ do, sι sι ka har hɛlɛlɛlɛ anι thɩ̃thιιn. Mɔ̃kɛ nιrɛ n haannι ɔɔ bιsã bisɔ hɛlɛlɛlɛ,
52002008	mɛ̃ sι kɔɔ ha nar ha lʋʋnna, a ƴaal ga-n do Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι sι-n ha nι dιbara ga, sι sι faa asι thɛthɛɛ yi anι sora, gιdonι nι lõ ser haar ka.
52002009	Omιna, mee nι jιnanɛ asι thɔ̃ do na asι vɔɔ; dιtιnɛ na dιwιlʋ sι-n kɔɔ do thɔma dι sa do heendaa tibil bιɛllalakɛ anι pa ga, thale sι kɔɔ mιι nar Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι.
52002010	Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛrakɛ kɔɔ to garɛ yire, na Thãgba dakha, dι nɛrɛɛkɛ pιɛrnι haar, sι hana narɛ cʋʋ pa bʋɔ, na fιl telẽe na dι pa 'leere.
52002011	Dι nι jιrɛ dakha mɔ̃kɛ thιrɛ n fʋnι ɔɔ bιsãsɔ, mɛ̃ sι kɔɔ fʋ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl bɔɔbɔɔ,
52002012	dι sa-n wɛ nι, dι sa-n ƴɔlna nι haar, dι sa-n fɛrɛna nι ayι: Na-n ιrɛ ga-n da Thãgbaraakɛ kɔɔ wɛ nιnι nι lona ɔɔ fãgadaar dora, a bulo kha na ɔɔ i dʋbι.
52002013	Gɛr dɔ kιrʋ dι sa-n khιι Thãgba wire fɛʋ, gιrɛraakɛ nι kɔɔ tuni Thãgbaa thιmιιkɛ sι kɔɔ mιι narnι, mɔ̃kɛ ga donι tibil thιmιιra', sιι do Thãgbaa thιmιι bʋɔ gι na sobɔr, dι ga-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ nɛrɛraakɛ pιɛrnι haar.
52002014	Gιdonι, nɛr omιna, nι debire a ha mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa we gbɛbιdaraakɛ dɔnι Jeju Kirisitii too, kɛ hanι Jude dιιra hanɩ, gaarɛraakɛ anɩ too n kɔɔ gaar nɩnɩ dɩɩ do bɩɛlla gɩ na gaarɛɛkɛ wɩrɛ dɔnɩ Juifisɔ n kɔɔ gaar wɩnɩ.
52002015	Juifisɔɔlera wɛr kɔɔ kɔ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn, na Thãgbaa bobonasɔ, wɛr kɔɔ kpoone sar dakha, awɩda na-n da Thãgba haara', wɩ-n laarɛ dakha tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
52002016	Wɛrra n pɩɛrɛ sɩ aa, sa-n mɩɩna ca kpala wɩ 'lɛ taara', dɩ thalera wɩ-n cʋʋ dɩ awɩ sopugo thʋ̃ ɩ̃ waa a dã thu, dɩɩ do waa Thãgba gbana wɛr nĩkhii khorr.
52002017	Sɩ ado sɛr wɛ omɩna, mɔ̃kɛ sɩ 'lee nɩnɩ gɩrɛ bɔɔ gbe tomɩrra sɩ ga do haarra ga, anɩ thu thʋnɛ fʋ sɩ waa ka, dɩ sa-n ƴaal ka sɩ yɛ nɩ kɔrɔ.
52002018	Mɛ̃ sɩ-n ƴaal gɩrɛ dɩphã sɩ pɔ anɩ pa, dɩ mɛr Polɩ thɛthɛ ƴaalɛlakɛ balanyɔ fɛʋ, sɩ Satã kɔɔ pɩɛr sɛr dɩ sa kɔɔ yɩ hʋɛa'.
52002019	Gɩdonɩ ʋmɔ̃ dɔrakɛ gɩrɛ asɩ nũ pɛ, agɩbo asɩ kãkada na asι khookɛ dɔnι i dʋbιdaa, ga do nɛr gι asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jejuu bir ɩ̃ bɔaa?
52002020	Ɔɔ, nɛr dɔ asι i dʋbιda na asι da.
52003001	Dι mɔ̃ sa-n marnι dιphã na too sa-n pιɛr mã', gɛr gι dι sι kɔɔ kpιɛr hιιn sa too dιbara Atɛn dιιra,
52003002	sa thɔ̃ Timothe asι omiikɛ dɔnι Thãgbaa thɔ̃ dodaar Kirisitii tutugo bɔ thιmιι mιιrɛra, a cʋɛ nɩ nɩ tɩ kɩbɩ, na-n yɩr anɩ ha pɛra.
52003003	Dɩ mɛ̃ tibil na hale a na jẽ kpooreraakɛ nɩ hanɩ gɩra', gɩdonɩ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ jɩrɛ sɩ hananɛ daa ser kpoorera.
52003004	Gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ hanɩ anɩ pa, sɩ kɔɔ mãa so nar dɩ sa yɩrɛ kpoore, dɩ gɩ kɔɔ daan otirə mɔ̃kɛ nɩ yɩɛnɩ.
52003005	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɔ̃ ma-n punoni dɩ ɩ̃ mar dɩ ɩ̃ toa', gɛr mɩ thʋɔn ɩ̃ jɩ mɔ̃ anɩ ha pɛ hanɩ, gɩdonɩ mɩ-n kɔɔ dɛr dɩ anaa Satãakɛ dɔnɩ fifilədaar na ba fɩɩl nɛ̃r gɩ ho mɔlɔ thɔma sɩ kɔɔ do.
52003006	Sɩ Timotheekɛ thɛnɩ anɩ pa a ɩ̃ gɩrɛ dɩ ga pʋɔra', ɔr mɩɛnɛ sɩ mɔ̃ anɩ ha pɛ hanɩ na anɩ naʋ dɩɩ da sar. A so sarɛ dakha dɩ wire fɛʋ nɩ-n hana jɩnanɛɛkɛ daanɔnɩ sɛrɛra, dɩ na-n ƴaal nɩ yɩ sɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ-n ƴaalnɩ sɩ yɩ nɩ.
52003007	Gɛr gɩ, omɩna, asɩ nɩ na kpoore fɛʋʋkɛ sɩ-n yɩnɩ, anɩ ha pɛ dor nɔɔ dɩ sɩ faa haar.
52003008	Nɛnɛ̃ mɩ fer waa fə̃ə, gɩdonɩ nɩ tɩrɛ kɩbɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra.
52003009	Mɔ̃ khɩɩrɛɛkɛ sa khɩɩnɩ Thãgba na thʋ̃ na ha kper anɩ sorara, na daʋ fɛʋraakɛ n fɔ sɩnɩ asɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra nɛrɛra.
52003010	Dɩtɩnɛ na dɩwɩlʋ sɩ-n bɩɛlʋʋ phãphãphã a hana sɩ hʋɛ sɩ yɩ nɩ, dɩ ka anɩ ha pɛ ɓɔrnɩ gɩ tɔ gɩ pɛr.
52003011	Thãgbaa thɛthɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Thɩ, na asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju n phɛla sɩ hʋɛ sɩ pɔ anɩ pa.
52003012	Sɩ ado nɛr gɩ, Kɔ̃tɩn n dɛ̃ɛ nar anɩ naʋʋkɛ nɩ hananɩ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl na tɩbɩla fɛʋra, gɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ga-n pɛr gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ asɩ naʋʋkɛ sɩ hana narnɩ hanɩ.
52003013	A cʋʋ nɩ nɩ tɩ, nɩ phu, na hana dɩ paar Thãgba asɩ Thɩɩ ƴɛra fɩɩʋraka', bɔɔkɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju na birni na ɩ̃ nakha ɔɔ tɩɩ phusɔ.
52004001	Ado gɩrɛ sɛnɩ gɩ omɩna, nɩ nɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ sɩ-n dɩɩr nɩnɩ dɩ gɩ teenanɛ na-n ɩrɛ ga-n da Thãgba haar, dɩɩ dorakɛ gɛr nɩ-n cʋʋ gɩrɛ, sɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr dɩ sa-n phʋʋrna nɩ na Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i, dɩ na-n ɩrɛ hʋɛrara na bãbar.
52004002	Nɩ jɩrɛ dakha mɔ̃ so ca ʋrɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ dɩ sɩ ha nɩ hanɩ.
52004003	Gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ gɛr dʋɔn anɩ kpɩɩ lee sopugora; gɛr dʋɔn nι hʋnɔnɛ na bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛ;
52004004	gɛr dʋɔn nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl n jɛ mɔ̃ na fʋnι anιbara, anι tomι n do daphuu, na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na hananɔnι cʋrɛ.
52004005	Dι na-n do thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛkɛ n hərəneni tibil na-n fʋ nι, mɔ̃kɛ gι-n hanι thιldararaakɛ na jɛnι Thãgba gaaga;
52004006	gɛr dʋɔn tibil na-n tagιrι ɔɔ omi, agιbo a na-n pιɛraa hara thιɛna ga, gιdonι Kɔ̃tιn na tiire helu ga thɩ̃sɔraale fɛʋ mɔ̃kɛ sι kɔɔ maanι so nar a kpãkpaanɔ.
52004007	Gιdonι Thãgba na kɔɔ we sι thɩ̃ bise cʋʋrɛra ga, sι sι pho.
52004008	Gɛr gι ʋrɛ bɔnι sorιkɛ ga do tibil a boa', sι Thãgba a bo, ʋrɛɛkɛ hana sιnι ɔɔ Thu Phuu.
52004009	Sι ado gιrɛ dɔnι omi naar gι, ma laar na khere nar dιkha bã, gιdonι Thãgbaa thɛthɛ dιrɛ nι ayι, na-n na khasɔ bιɛlbιɛl.
52004010	Dι gɛrra dɔrakɛ gιrɛ nι-n cʋʋnι gɩrɛ omɩnasɔra fɛʋʋkɛ hanι Masedʋan dιιra koo, sι sι-n phʋʋr nɛr omɩna, dɩ na jɩɩ bãba gɩ jɔ mɛ̃.
52004011	Nɩ yɩra a tɔɔ mʋmʋr, na-n jɩɛ ɔ anɩ thɩ̃sɔra bɔɔbɔɔ, na-n gbuo yʋʋ anɩ nyɛ̃kɩɛr thɔna, mɔ̃kɛ sɩ kɔɔ dɩɩr nɩnɩ.
52004012	Dɩ mɛ̃ na hana fɩlɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ wɩrɛ na dɔnɩ ha pɛdara gaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, gɩ do nɔɔ dakha na too na-n therna tibilə'.
52004013	Omɩna, ado wɩrɛ daarɛnɩ daanɩkɛ dɔnɩ khir gɩ, sa-n ƴaal na-n jɩ mɔ̃ gɩ hanaa ga, na-n bɩ nɩ ho wɛkɛ na hananɩ nũ pɛraa ga.
52004014	Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ sɩ pɛrnɩ haar gel dɩ Jeju kɔɔ khire sa bir a ɩɩr a the khirera, mɛ̃ sɩ jɩ dakha ga har na wɩrɛ pɩɛrnɩ Jeju haar sa daar, Thãgba na kpa wɛr dɩ wa ɩ̃ kha na Jeju.
52004015	Nɩ yɛ gɩrɛ sɩ-n mɩɩ nɩnɩ mɔ̃kɛ Kɔ̃tɩn sonɩ, sɛr yidaraakɛ na sɛnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ ɩ̃ bɔɔ, wɩrɛɛkɛ daarɛnɩ daanɩkɛ dɔnɩ khir sa kɔɔ kʋʋl wɩ ƴɩɛ a na jʋʋna'.
52004016	Gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɛthɛ na ther Thãgbaa dʋɔ a na-n gbũ, dɩ nɔ khɩɩr na phaan, wa nɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ nɔ, dɩ dakha Thãgbaa tutuu na ʋnɛ, le wɩrɛ pɩɛrnɩ Kirisiti haar sa khiir na kɔɔ ɩɩr cacaca a na the khirera.
52004017	Agɩpɩ dɩphã sɛr yidaraakɛ na sɛnɩ, Thãgba na və̃ ser kha na wɛr dɩ sa gbɛbɩ kha kãkɛ ndɔlɔ̃pana hanɩ, gɩ do le sɩ caan Kɔ̃tɩn thãgbara ƴũ. Mɛ̃ na dɔ asɩ too sa toonɩ kha waa khorr na Kɔ̃tɩn.
52004018	Gɛr gɩ nɩ gba thɩmɩaakɛra a na ƴɔlana kha haar bɩɛlbɩɛl.
52005001	Sɩ omɩna, ado bɔɔkɛ ga donɩ wer na wireekɛ ga donɩ, ma laar na khere nar ga thɩmɩa',
52005002	gɩdonɩ nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛrakɛ jɩɛ jɩ dɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wi na daan mɔ̃ yu n ɩnɩ dɩtɩnɔ.
52005003	Ɔbɔɔkɛ tɩbɩla na sonɩ nayι: Ha ιι hale; wo: Thɩ̃ɛ bɔrɛ dιphã waa. Liir bũburone na phuro wi dapaara mɔ̃ wallɛ n phũroni khɛ pɛmɛdaar, gι do wa yι for paar bã.
52005004	Sι ne wer omιna, na ha dabirəra Wi caale n phuroni mɔ̃ yu n phuronə'.
52005005	Nɛrɛ fɛʋ, nɛr dʋɔn dahιrɛdara na dιwιldara, sa ha kha dιkha na dιtɩnɛ dɩ dabirə ga.
52005006	Dɩ gɛr gɩ sa-n daar wɛɛ kha ga, sɩ sa-n jʋrɛ a hanana dakha dɩbara fʋrɛ.
52005007	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n daarɛnɩ dɩtɩnɔ wɩ-n daar, dɩ wɩrɛ taan n kʋnɩ dɩtɩnɔ gɩ-n kʋ wɩ.
52005008	Sɩ sɛrkɛ dɔnɩ dɩwɩldara sɩ hanana dɩbara fʋrɛ, a dɔ wɩrɛ tʋɔnnɩ ha pɛrɛ na naʋ kũkũ kɛɛ the khaa, a subo dakha taa 'lɛ nũ pɛrɛ the kpɛ khaa.
52005009	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba na kɔɔ thɩɩn sɩ sɩ lona ɔɔ nĩkhirə ga, sɩ sɩ 'lɛ taarɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitira,
52005010	kɛ kɔɔ khe sarnɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ ado sɩ hananɛ yire, ado sɩ daarɛ, sɩ sa hananɛ kha yire na ɔr.
52005011	Gɛr gɩ na-n mɩa kha yɩr thɩmɩa bɩɛlbɩɛ̃l, ʋ n tɔ ʋ a na-n jalna ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ-n cʋʋnɩ gɩrɛ.
52005012	Omɩna, sɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr dɩ na hana cʋrɛ wɩrɛraakɛ n gbũgbuloneni anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, kɛ dɔnɩ anɩ ƴɛ kʋʋldara, dɩ wa-n dɩɩr nɩ fɩlɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ hʋra.
52005013	Na-n cɔ wɩ dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na naʋʋkɛ hanɩ phãphãphã gɩ do awɩ thɔ̃ dɔ nɔɔ. Na-n tɔ̃ɔ kha na ha ɩɩ.
52005014	Sɩ-n phʋʋr nɛr dakha omɩna, na-n kpãkpaanɛ khãkhalala, na-n hana ha phaadara 'lar, na-n bulo wɩrɛ yɔɔnɩ, na-n hana ha fʋrɛ na tɩbɩla fɛʋ.
52005015	Na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn dɩ a tibil cʋʋ ʋ̃ tibil puure a na-n bir lɩmʋʋ puurə', sɩ bɔɔ fɛʋ anɩ hara na tɩɩ kpɩɩsɔra fɛʋ, na-n yɩrana bɔ cʋʋrɛ.
52005016	Na-n hana daʋ wire fɛʋ.
52005017	Na-n bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba tɔ̃tɔ̃tɔ̃.
52005018	Na-n fʋɔrɛ Thãgba thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra a gɩ ha mɔ̃, gɩdonɩ gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ anɩ pa, nɛrkɛ hanɩ Jeju Kirisitira.
52005019	Na-n khiir Thu Phuu dɔa'.
52005020	Na-n beesi Thãgba tukɩr tirə',
52005021	sɩ nɩ mɩɛnɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na hɩnɛ, sɩ na fʋɔr gɩrɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ.
52005022	Nɩ hʋnɔnɛ na thɩ̃ puu caar dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ.
52005023	Thãgbaakɛ ha ɩɩ n thernɩ, ɔɔ thɛthɛ n lea nɩ kpɩɩ koo nɩ phu, dɩ anɩ thɛthɛɛ tɩɩ dorakɛ koo: Thue, na haar, na tomɩr n jɩɩ too gɩ 'lee dɩ paar, gɩ dana wireekɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na birni na ɩ̃.
52005024	Ʋrɛɛkɛ wɛ nɩnɩ sobɔdaar a dõ, dι ɔrra dakha na cʋɛ gι.
52005025	Omιna, nι bιɛlnɛ Thãgba na pɛ sar.
52005026	Nι fʋɔrɛ omιna fɛʋ na ha lõ fʋɔrɛ.
52005027	Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i mι gba dɩ ma-n kpãkpaana nar, nɩ sɔ sɛbɛɛkɛ omɩna fɛʋ n nɩɛ.
52005028	Asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ nɩ bʋɔra.
53001001	Mɛr Pol na Sɩlvɛ̃ na Timothe thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha we gbɛbɩdaraakɛ hanɩ Tesalonɩkɩ, kɛ Thãgba asɩ Thɩ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn hɩnɩ.
53001002	Thãgba Thɩrɛ na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩn n hana nɩ ha ɩɩ a jɛ nɩ dakha bʋɔra.
53001003	Omιna, asιda dʋɔn dɔ sa-n khιι Thãgba wire wire anιdara, dι gι teenanɛ dι sa cʋʋ mɛ̃ gιdonι anι ha pɛra kɔ̃tιnɛ dι ga-n pɛr, dι anι naʋʋkɛ nι-n nanι kha bιɛlbιɛl dakha gι-n dɛɛnɔnɛ.
53001004	Dι gι dor nɔɔ dι sɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ na-n məbi anιdara, Thãgbaa we gbɛbιdarasɔɔ thɩ̃thιιn, gιdonι anι kιbι jιιl dɔ nɔɔ, na anι ha pɛɛkɛ nι hananιnakɛ kpoore na bɔ gaarɛra fɛʋʋkɛ nι-n yιnιι thɩ̃thιιn.
53001005	Gɛr n nɛna Thãgbaa kιιl sar, gι do nɔɔ gι do nι teenanɛ lʋʋn Thãgbaa fãgadaar dora, kɛra nι-n gaarɔnι bʋɔ mɛ̃.
53001006	Gιdonι Thãgba sarrɛ gɛr a na gbaar bɔ gaarɛ ana lιmι wιrɛ n gaarɛ nιnι,
53001007	dι nɛrɛɛkɛ wι-n gaarnι gιrɛ, a na gbaar hιιrɛ a na ha nι nakha sɛrɛ dakha, ɔbɔɔkɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tιn na thenι Thãgbaa dʋɔ a na-n ɩ̃ gbelẽ gbelẽ na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ na fãga,
53001008	na dɔlιnanɛ. A na tiire helu wιrɛraakɛ na jɛnι Thãgba ga, na wιrɛraakɛ na-n nɛnι asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jejuu tutugo bɔ thɩmɩɩ nũə'.
53001009	Awɩ so heen na dor bũburone khorr, wɩ hʋnɔnanɩ Kɔ̃tɩn a 'leena ɔɔ fãgaakɛ thɛnɩ ɔɔ puno hanana.
53001010	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Wireelera na danɩ a na-n ɩ̃ kpãgarɛ na-n ther ɔɔ tɩɩ phusɔɔ pa, wɩrɛ fɛʋ pɩɛrnɩ haar na hananaanɛ cʋʋr, dɩ nɛrkɛ pɩɛrnɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ haar na harrɛ ner.
53001011	Gɛr gɩ dakha dɩ sɩ bɩɛl Thãgba bɔɔ fɛʋ dɩ sa-n pɛ nar, asɩ Thãgba n cʋɛ nɩ nɩ teena ɔɔ wera, a gba ɔɔ fãga a cʋʋna nɩ nɩ puno na-n cʋʋ bɔɔkɛ nι-n ƴaalnι, a cʋʋna anι ha pɛ thɩ̃ cʋʋ ga-n dã otirə.
53001012	Dι mɛ̃ na do nɔɔ dι asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jejuu i na 'lɛ kpãgarɛ, dι na 'lɛr dakha kpãgarɛ gι do ɔr dɔ nɔɔ, gι the asι Thãgba na asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii bɔ jιra.
53002001	Sι-n bιɛl nɛr omιna, ado gιrɛ dɔnι asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii bir ɩ̃da gι, na asι gbɛbι kha na ɔr,
53002002	na-n do kpιɛrɛ nyanyãa nι kɔrɔa', dι na-n do dakha haar na-n jɛ̃ nι gιrɛraakɛ tibil na yιnι aa, Thu Phuu mιana nɩ agɩbo thɩmɩɩr ɩnɩ nɩ agɩbo aa, sɛbɛ thɛ asɩ pa ayɩ, Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wi daan pa'.
53002003	A gɩ ha mɔnakɛ na-n do tibil n fɩɩl na', gɩdonɩ dɔ Thãgba so bʋʋrɛ n kɔɔ ɩ̃ ɓo wɩ yɩ Sopugo tibilile a yɩr, kɛ wɩ thɩɩnnɩ bũburõ thɩɩnʋʋ,
53002004	Thãgbaa vardaar gɩɩkɛ na ɩrɛnɩ na yʋ bʋʋn gɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Thãgba na gɩrɛraakɛ tibil n fʋɔrnɩ, a ba toorakɛ Thãgba fʋɔr cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna sɩ ayɩ, ɩnɛrɛɛ thɛthɛra dɔ Thãgbara.
53002005	Na jιna mɔ̃ mι-n kɔɔ mιɛ nιnι ga thɩ̃ιlera ɔbɔɔkɛ mι kɔɔ hanι anι pa gaa?
53002006	Dι nɛnɛ̃ nι jιrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ pιɛrɛɛnι dι agado bɔɔ dana ga hʋɛ na yιr da tha'.
53002007	Gιdonι fãga gbulikɛ dɔnι sopugodaa 'lire har dι ga-n do thɔma, foo ʋrɛ pιɛrɛɛnι nɛnɛ̃ n tɔ a khokhιa ɓo dιphã.
53002008	Liir Sopugodaarιlera na yιr dι wa yιι, kɛ Jeju Kɔ̃tιn na phʋʋnι na kʋ, a na hɛlʋʋlɛ dι ɔɔda na ther mɔ̃ a na-n ιnι ga-n carbara.
53002009	Sopugodaarι ɩ̃ιle Satãa fãgara ga the, na nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ, na jιιnsɔ, na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔ, dι gelesɔ fɛʋra na jɔrɛ na ka a na do tιι fιιldaa.
53002010	A na gbaar gιrɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ puu caar dιιdιι fɛʋ a na-n fιιlna wιrɛ n buureni, gιdonι wa na sobɔr a na 'lɛ taara'.
53002011	Gɛrra dɔ kιrʋ dι Thãgba thɔna war fãga ga-n fιιl wι wa-n pɛr sõsor haar.
53002012	Dι mɛ̃ wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na pιɛrnι sobɔr haara', sιι do thɩ̃ puu ka da war, na 'lɛ kιιlʋ.
53002013	Sι ado sɛr wɛ, omιnaakɛ Kɔ̃tιn n nanι, sι teenanɛ sa-n khιa Thãgba wire wire anι sora, gιdonι Thãgba kɔɔ phire ni caca fʋ paar dι na 'lɛ taarɛ, gι the Thu Phuurəəkɛ lea nιnι kpιι, gι the dakha ha pɛrɛraakɛ nι pɛrnι sobɔr haar.
53002014	Gɛr dɔ gιrɛ a gbarɔnι tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ sι-n mιιnι a wena nι, nι puno nι bul kha na asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii i dʋbɩ.
53002015	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ omɩna, nɩ fɔ gɩ ma, nɩ fɔ dɩɩrɛɛkɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ, ado na asɩ nɔ gɩ, ado na asɩ sɛbɛsɔ gɩ.
53002016	Dɔ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii thɛthɛ, na Thãgba asɩ Thɩ, kɛ kɔɔ naan sɩnɩ, kɛ kɔɔ hana sɩnɩ khorr ha faarɛ na nũ pɛ bʋɔ bɔ jɩɩrra,
53002017	n cʋʋ nɩ na-n faa haar, a cʋʋ nι dakha nι 'lɛ fãga thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛra fɛʋ na thιmιι bɔιra fɛʋ.
53003001	Gιrɛ sɛnɩ omɩna, nɩ bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba na pɛ sar Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩ n puno gɩ ca ga-n kpaar ga-n 'lɛ cʋʋr, mɔ̃kɛ gɩ hanɩ gɩrɛ anɩ pa;
53003002	gɩ do nɔɔ dakha Thãgba n taa sɩ gõgolõdarara na tɩɩ puusɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ, gɩdonɩ ga do tɩbɩla fɛʋ hana ha pɛra'.
53003003	Sɩ sobɔdaar Kɔ̃tɩn do, ɔr gɩɩkɛ na cʋɛ nɩnɩ dɩ na tɩ kɩbɩ, a na bɛr nɛr dakha puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarra.
53003004	Dɩrakɛ sɩ hana narɛ ha pɛrɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnna, dɩ gɩrɛ sɩ kɔɔ so narnɩ nɩ-n cʋʋrɛ, dɩ thalera na cʋʋrakɛ na-n jalna.
53003005	Kɔ̃tɩn n thɔɔ anɩ ha a na pɛ naʋraakɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaada na Kirisitii ha fʋra.
53003006	Asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii i sι gba dι sa-n kpãkpaana nar omιna, dι na hʋnɔ kha na omine wo omineekɛ dɔnι khãkhal, kɛ na-n ιrɛnι mɔ̃kɛ dιιrɛɛkɛ nι kɔɔ 'lɛnι asι pa hana'.
53003007	Nɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ jιrɛ anιbara mɔ̃kɛ gι teenanι nι phɛla sι, gιdonι ɔbɔɔkɛ sι kɔɔ hanι anι pa sa do khãkhala ga.
53003008	Sa kɔɔ kho tibili dιko sι sa lιmaa ga, sι dιtιnɛ na dιwιlʋ sι-n kɔɔ do thɔ̃ khena na vɔɔrɛ dι sa do heendaa tibil bιɛllalakɛ anι pa ga.
53003009	Sɩ ga do hʋɛ sa kɔɔ hana gaaga, sɩ thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ sɩ ƴaal sɩ do nar na-n phɛl sɩ.
53003010	Gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ hanɩ anɩ pa sɩ-n kɔɔ kpãkpãa narɛ ayɩ: Tibilikɛ n bɔnɩ thɔ̃ dʋʋr aa hana hʋɛ na kho dɩkor dakha ga.
53003011	Sɩ sɩ nɩɛrɛ dɩ ɩkhasɔ har anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a do khãkhala, wa-n do thɔma ga, sɩ dɩ wa-n hɩɩn gɩrɛ na ba wɩna'.
53003012	Ado wa tibil casɔɔle wɛ, sɩ gba Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩnɩ i a na kpãkpaana wɩ a tɔna wɩ na pɩɛr wa-n dɔ awɩ thɔ̃ mʋmʋr, a yɛ awɩ nyɛ̃kɩɛr thɩ̃ɩkɛ na-n haanɛ wɩnɩ.
53003013	Sɩ ado nɛr wɛ omɩna, na-n vɔɔ bɔ cʋʋrɛra ga.
53003014	Sɩ ado tibil na-n nɩ thɩmɩaakɛ sɩ kherenɩ sɛbɛraakɛ nũə', nɩ dʋɔraa bʋrɛ, na-n bɔ kha na tibil ca ola', gɩ do nɔɔ yicuru n fʋʋ.
53003015	Sɩ na-n hɩɩnʋʋ lãlaar hɩɩnʋa', sɩ na-n dɩrɛɛ omi dɩɩrɛ.
53003016	Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ ha ɩɩ n thernɩ, ɔɔ thɛthɛ na-n ha nɩ ha ɩɩ bɔɔ fɛʋ, thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra. Kɔ̃tɩn na-n hana kha na nɛrɛ fɛʋ.
53003017	Mɛr Pol khera fʋɔrɛɛkɛ na ɩ̃ nyɛ̃. Gɛr dɔ jɩɩn ɩ̃ sɛbɛsɔra fɛʋ, thale dɔ ɩ̃ khere.
53003018	Asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra.
54001001	Mɛr Polɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn, dɩɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Taadaar pɛrnɩ gɩ hana, na Jeju Kirisitiikɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ sɩ-n pɛnɩ nũu,
54001002	thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Timotheekɛ dɔ marnι bikuun na sobɔr ha pɛdaara: Thãgba Thιrɛ, na asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ fɩ bʋɔra, a na-n dɔna fɩ dakha bʋɔ, a na-n hana fɩ dakha ha ɩɩ.
54001003	Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ-n gbanɩ hʋɛ ɩ̃ jal Masedʋan, mɩ kɔɔ so farɛ fɩ tɔɔ Efɛjɩ a vara kĩkĩ tibil ɩkhasɔra wa-n dɩɩr sõso dɩɩra'.
54001004	Wa-n bo na pɛ dakha kpuro nɩɛsɔ nũə', na thɩ kɔ̃ jɔfʋsɔa', kɛ ga thɩmɩɩ na-n hananɩ khu paara ga, sɩɩ do kɩla gɩ-n ɩɩr, sɩ ga-n ka cʋʋ gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ ga-n cʋɛa', gɩdonɩ ha pɛrɛra gele n cʋʋ.
54001005	Gɩrɛ Thãgbaa so 'laa n ƴaalnɩ ga-n cʋɛ dʋɔn gɩ dɔ naʋ a na thɛ ha phuurə, na kpɩɛrnɔraakɛ 'leanɩ dɩ paar, na ha pɛrɛraakɛ na hananɩ fɩɩla'.
54001006	Ɩkhasɔ kɔɔ dɩrɛ hʋɛra, a lɛ̃, a lõ mɔlɔ thɩ̃ banaana;
54001007	sɩ wɩ-n ƴaalɛ ɩnɩ-n dɔ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdara, sɩrakɛ gɩrɛ wɩ-n sonɩ wa-n jɩ ga kɩra', dɩ thɩmɩɩ nɔ ʋrɛ wɩ-n bonɩ wa-n ɩɩrɔ, wa jɩ ɔɔ kɩr dakha ga.
54001008	Sɩ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ jɔfʋ bɔrɛ a fɩ jɩ mɔ̃ na mɔ̃ gɩ teenanɩ fɩ cʋɛnaa,
54001009	a fɩ jɩ dɩɩ do ga do tɩɩ sarʋra jɔfʋ kɔɔ pɛra', sι jɔfʋ 'leedarara wɛ, na nũ nʋʋrdarara, na wɩrɛraakɛ na-n therananɩ Thãgba ga, na sopugodarara, na Thãgba fʋɔr bodarara, na Thãgba so ƴɔ̃ƴɔ̃ɔdarara, na thɩ kʋdarara, na nɩ kʋdarara, na tɩɩ kʋdarara,
54001010	na bɔdɛl cʋʋdarara, na konanaakɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ kuun khɛr khaa, na khɛraraakɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ khɛr kũu khaa, na tɩɩ dolõdarara, na sõsodarara, na sõso ʋlfɛdarara, na gɩrɛ fɛʋraakɛ n varanɩ dɩɩr bɔ.
54001011	Dɩɩrɛɛlera tutugo bʋɔraakɛ Thãgba pɛ marnɩ dɩ ma mɩɩ, le gɩ the; dɩ tutugo bʋɔ gɩɩkɛ n nɛnanɩ mɔ̃ Thãgbaakɛ hɩnanɩ i dʋbɩrɛ a hɩna bɔnanɛ hanɩ.
54001012	Mɩ-n khɩɩrɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ hana mɩnɩ fãga, kɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisiti asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃, na gιrɛraakɛ a we mɩnɩ sobɔ tibil a gba mɩ pɛ thɔmana,
54001013	mɛrkɛ mamara kɔɔ dɔnɩ ɔɔ i kʋɛdaar, na kpõkpoodaar, na nĩkhi khedaar, sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ mɛr bʋɔra, gɩdonɩ yʋ 'leerera na ha pɛ 'leerera mι kɔɔ cʋʋ gelela.
54001014	Asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ nɩna mɛr ɔɔ bɔ jɩ dɩɩ thʋ̃ kãasɩ, a hanana mɩ ha pɛrɛ na naʋʋkɛ thɛnɩ Jeju Kirisitira.
54001015	Sobɔr thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ do a teena tuur koo, gɛr dʋɔn Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ ɩnɛ kɛ thɩɩra a taa sopugodara, kɛ mɛrɛ donɩ cacadaar.
54001016	Sɩ Thãgba kɔɔ jɩ mɛr bʋɔra, gɩ do mɛr dɔ cacadaarɩkɛ Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ nɩrɔnɩ ɔɔ ha fʋ koo, ɩ̃ do thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ wɩrɛraakɛ na pɩɛnɩ haar a na 'lɛ yire khorr.
54001017	Ʋrɛ dɔnι bɔɔ khorr fãgadaar, kɛ na dɔnι dakhinənə', aa do wo dayιnana', kɛ dɔnι Thãgba bιɛl dιbara 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ, ɔr teana a hιna cʋrɛ na i dʋbιrɛ bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
54001018	Mι gbaar sorɩkɛ dɩ ma-n ha fɛr Timothe ɩ̃ bikuun, mɔ̃kɛ Thãgbaa bobonaa thɩmɩɩkɛ telene fɩnɩ kɔɔ maanɩ sor, gba gɩ a na kɛ̃kɛrɛna kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ bʋɔ,
54001019	a jɩɛ hanana ha pɛrɛ na kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ na heene fɩnɩ sora'; ga kpɩɛrnɔ caalera ɩkhasɔ kɔɔ dʋna gɛr a faa a kʋɛ awɩ ha pɛ;
54001020	Imene na Alesãdɩɩr kɔɔ harrɛ, dɩ mɩ kɔɔ faa wɛr a ha Satã gɩ dɩɩr wɩ fɩlɛ wɩ faa Thãgbaa i kʋɛrɛ.
54002001	Dɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ caca thɩ̃ɛ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ dʋɔn, phʋʋrɛ, na bɩɛlɛ, na ƴɛɛrɛ, na Thãgba khɩɩrɛ, sa-n pɛ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ.
54002002	Sɩ bɩɛlnɛ a na pɛ fãgadarara fɛʋ na wɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩnasɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ sa too dɩɩra cɔcɔcɔ na ha ɩɩ, sɩ hana Thãgba fɩlɛ na fɩl bʋɔ;
54002003	thale bʋɔnɔ, gɛr n da dakha Thãgbaraakɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Taadaar,
54002004	kɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n 'lɛ taarɛ a jɛ gɩrɛ n dɔnɩ sobɔr.
54002005	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba bɩɛl dɩbara haanle, na dakha so ƴɛɛdaar bɩɛl tɩbɩlala na Thãgba, Jeju Kirisitiikɛ dɔnɩ tibil gɩ.
54002006	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ faanɩ dɩbara a birse tɩbɩla fɛʋ, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ ga bɔɔlera kɔɔ danɩ gɩ har mɔna gɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ.
54002007	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Thãgba pɛ marnɩ dɩ ɩ̃ do ga mɩmɩɩ na thɔ̃thɔn, ma-n dɩɩr ca kpala ha pɛrɛ, na gɩrɛ dɔnɩ sobɔr, dɩ sobɔr mɩ-n so ga do sõsor mɩ kurə'.
54002008	Dɩ gɛr gɩ mɩ-n ƴaalɛ kona n 'laanɛ nyɛ̃ phuu ƴũ a na bιɛlna Thãgba paar fɛʋ, sι wa-n hana nĩkhiə', wa-n hana thɩ̃ banaa ga.
54002009	Mι-n ƴaalɛ dakha khɛra na-n tɔ kẽkena mɔ̃kɛ gι teenanι, na fɩl bʋɔ na fιl phuu, wa-n li yʋʋ dι yʋ lιιr gɩ, a gbana dɛ thɩ̃ɛsɔ na lẽbiisɔ na kẽkẽ the nɔ khena ka, a na cʋʋna biirə';
54002010	sɩ gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ awɩ biir cʋʋ n ka dɔ thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛ, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ teananɩ khɛraakɛ n yɛnι Thãgba cʋ khɛra ιnɩ do.
54002011	Dɔ khɛra n 'wɩɩ kɩrkɩrkɩr sɩ wa-n pɛ dɩɩrɛ nũu na dɩbara jor.
54002012	Ma-n tu khɛr n dɔ dɩɩrdaara', agɩbo a do yʋʋ kuunna ga, sɩ a teenanɛ a 'wɩa kɩrkɩrkɩr.
54002013	Gɩdonɩ Adã Thãgba kɔɔ ti ɓo sa pιιrɔ Ɛvɩ.
54002014	Sɩ ga do Adã kɔɔ telene a 'lɛ fifiləla', sι khɛr kɔɔ 'lɛ fifiləle a lõ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ kʋɛrɛra.
54002015	Sɩrakɛ Thãgba na tagʋʋrɛ mɔ̃ a donɩ bi kɔn, ado a too a hana fɩl phuu ɔɔ ha pɛra, na naʋra, na kpɩɩ leerera.
54003001	Sobɔr thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ do gɩ yɩ: Ado tibil na ɩnɩ-n dɔ we gbɛbɩdaraa hɩɩndaar thɔ̃ bʋɔ a-n ƴaal.
54003002	Dɩ gɛr gɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa hɩɩndaar teenanɛ a dɔ ʋrɛ tibil na punoni na pɛr sora' a hanana khɛ bɩɛl, a dɔ dɩbara fʋdaar, a dɔ yʋ bɔ tibil, a hanana fɩl bʋɔ, a dɔ kpakpal tee tibil, a punone a na dɩrɛ tibil thɩ̃ɛ;
54003003	a na-n do ta laardaara', a na-n do kɩl ƴaal tibilə', sɩ a dɔ bɩ̃ bɔ tibil, na ha ie ƴaal tibil, a na-n do war laardaara'.
54003004	Dɔ a do tibilikɛ n punoneni da-n ma ɔɔ cɔra, dɩ jɩɩ fʋ ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ dɩ wa-n nɩ nũu dɩ wɩ hananaa cʋʋr.
54003005	Gɩdonɩ ado tibil na puno a na ma ɔɔ cɔra ga, mɔ̃ a na fʋ sɩ na ma Thãgbaa we gbɛbɩdarara?
54003006	Sɩ wo ntɛ na-n do Thãgbadaar phaa ga, anaa a na kar ire a na ba lõ so heen ca bɩɛlla na Satã.
54003007	Sɩ a dɔ tibilikɛ hananɩ i bʋɔ wɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ ha pɛdara ga, dɩ mɛ̃ tibil na yɩɩraa so paara', a na ji dakha Satãa pherra ga.
54003008	Mɛna gɩ ha dakha na wɩrɛ dɔnɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa thɔ̃ dodara, wɩ teenanɛ wɩ dɔ tɩɩ cʋnanɛ, wa-n do khalƴιɛ yenyɔdara ga, wa-n do ta laardara ga, wa-n phʋʋn tɩbɩla na fãga bɩɩ awɩ war ƴaalla ga,
54003009	wɩ jɩɛ ma thɩ̃ gbulləəkɛ dɔnɩ ha pɛrɛɛda, a hanana kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ 'leanɩ dɩ paar.
54003010	Wa jʋʋr wɛr ɓo na hɩɩn ado wa hana so paara' wa-n do awɩ thɔ̃.
54003011	Ɔmɛna gɩ dakha na khɛra, wɩ teenanɛ wɩ dɔ tɩɩ cʋnanɛ, wa-n do i kʋɛ tibilə', wɩ hana dɩbara fʋrɛ, wɩ dɔ sobɔ cʋʋ tɩbɩla thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
54003012	We gbɛbɩdaraa thɔ̃ dodara teenanɛ wɩ hanana khɛ bɩɛl, wɩ jɩɛ ma awɩ bɩsãsɔra na awɩ thɛthɛɛ cɔra.
54003013	Gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n jɩɛnnɩ do awɩ thɔ̃ bɔɔbɔɔ, wɩ-n tɔr awɩ thɛthɛɛ cʋ dɩ wa-n pɛr, dɩ wɩ hananɛ dakha 'lar ha pɛrɛraakɛ wɩ hananɩ Jeju Kirisitira.
54003014	Mι khere farɛ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ sι mι pɛrɛ haar kιɛr na gbe ma pɔr afι pa.
54003015	Dι ado ma pʋɔr sι fι jι mɔ̃ tibil teenanι ɔɔ fιl n hana Thãgbaa too thɩ̃thιιn, kɛ dɔnι dakha Thãgba yidaarι we gbɛbιdara, a dona thιkarʋ ka sobɔr dɛɛnι.
54003016	Tibil na puno na bana mɔ̃ Thãgba fʋɔrɛ donι thɩ̃ hulõo a ka ga, gɛr dʋɔn: Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ gbaar tibil tomιr a debi do tιι yιnanɛ, Thu Phuu kɔɔ nιrɔrɛ dι tιι sarʋ a do; thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ kɔɔ yιιrɛ. Ɔɔda kɔɔ mιιrɛ casι tibil caarsɔra; wι kɔɔ pιɛrɛ haar thιιraakɛ, Thãgba kɔɔ khəsuure dι 'lɛ i dʋbιrɛ le ƴũ.
54004001	Thu Phuu sor casι ayι: Pιpιι bɔɔ ιkhasɔ na-n pɛr kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔda nũu, kɛ na cʋɛ wιnι wι buur, wι faana ha pɛrɛ gι the kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ dιιrraalera.
54004002	Sõsodaraakɛ daanɔnι nʋɔ, kɛ haar dibini mɔ̃ wι-n fɔfɔrɔnι haar na the phʋɛ, na fιlɛ wι nayι,
54004003	tibil na-n he khɛr dι kuun ga; aa, wa-n sãsιnɛ dakha thɩ̃ khonanɛɛkɛ Thãgba tini, dι wιrɛ dɔnɩ ha pɛdara a jɩna sobɔr na kho na fɔfʋɔr haar.
54004004	Gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ Thãgba tini gɩ bɔrɛ, thɩ̃ bonanɛ na hala', sɩ gɩ dor gɩrɛ tibil na fʋɔrɔnɩ Thãgba sɩ a na-n tee;
54004005	gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ na Thãgba bɩɛlɛ n cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ phu.
54004006	Ado fɩ gba ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ a na dɩɩr omɩna, ga dor fɩ dor Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃daar bʋɔɔkɛ ha pɛ thɩmɩɩr n haannɩ na dɩɩr bʋɔ, kɛ dakha fɩ kparɔnɩ bɔɔbɔɔ.
54004007	Bɔ mama sɔɔkɛ hɔnɩ kpuro nɩɛ, sɩ na gbuoro yʋʋ Thãgba fɩlɛla.
54004008	Gɩdonɩ tomɩ gbʋ̃gbʋnyanɛ wer, dabʋɔ harrɛ gbe, sɩ Thãgba fɩl hananɛ, dabʋɔ harrɛ a thʋ̃ kãasɩ, gɩdonɩ gɩ-n ɩnanɛ nɛnɛ̃ yire na yireekɛ na ɩnanɩ ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ.
54004009	Sobɔr thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ do a teena tuur koo.
54004010	Gɛr gɩ dɩ sa-n gbũgbulõ thɔmana dɩ sa-n kɛ̃kɛrɛna gɩ, gɩdonɩ asɩ nũ pɛ Thãgba yidaarra gɩ ha, kɛ dɔnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ Taadaar, sι ha pɛdaraa Taadaar a do cacaca.
54004011	Na kpãkpaanɛ war ga thɩ̃ιkɛ a na dιrɛna wɩ.
54004012	Tibil na-n beesi lι daɓol dʋʋrra ga, sɩ ka dɔ thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ ha pɛdarara, thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛra na cʋʋ paarra, na naʋra, na ha pɛrɛra, na phurrə.
54004013	Gɩ dana bɔɔkɛ ma pɔnɩ le, gbuoro yʋʋ a na sɔ sɛbɛ, a na mɩa Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ, a na dɩrɛna tɩbɩla.
54004014	Fa-n hɛbɩ bɔ jɩ khaardaakɛ ha farnɩ, kɛ fɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ dɩɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba tukɩr tidara kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ bɔɔraakɛ we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ dɛ̃ɛ farnɩ nyɛ̃a'.
54004015	Na jɩɛ tɩrɔ ga thɩ̃ɩle; faa afɩbara gɛrra, dɩ mɛ̃ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na yɩ mɔ̃ fɩ-n bãbanɩ.
54004016	Na jɩɛ hɩɩn afɩbara, na afɩ dɩɩr, na yɩrana ga thɩ̃ɩle; gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ fa-n cʋʋnɩ thalera fa taarɛ afɩbara na wɩrɛɛkɛ n pɛ fɩnɩ nũu.
54005001	Fa-n phaan kũu kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ na fɩlɛɛkɛ khiinona', sɩ mɩanaa mɔ̃ a donɩ thɩrɛ; fɔ daɓola õkũu khaa,
54005002	na khɛ kɔ̃tɩna nɩ khaa, na khɛ biirə õkhɛ̃ khaa, sɩ dɔ gɩ do na fɩl phuu.
54005003	Wɩrɛ dɔnɩ khikhɛra na sobɔr, na jɩɛ hɩɩn wɩ.
