54005004	Sɩ a khikhɛrʋ gι a hana bɩsana, agɩbo ɔɔ bii bɩsãsɔ gɩ, dɔ wɩ jɩ dɩ caca thɩ̃ɛ Thãgba fʋɔrɛra dʋɔn awɩ cɔdaraa hɩɩn, dɩ wa tiir dakha helu wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ haanɛ wɩnɩ, gɩdonɩ gɛr dʋɔn thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n danɩ Thãgba haar.
54005005	Sɩ ʋrɛ dɔnɩ khikhɛrʋ na sobɔr, aa hana tibil bã, Thãgba a-n pɛ nũu; dɩtɩnɔ na dɩwɩlʋ a-n yɩr da-n phʋʋr Thãgba da-n bɩɛlnaa.
54005006	Sɩ khikhɛrʋʋkɛ n faanɩ dɩbara da-n 'lɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ n daaraanɩ khaakhaar cʋʋrɛra, fɩ-n yɩɩrɛ na yire wer sɩ a khire.
54005007	Na kpãkpaanɛ war thɩ̃ɛsɔra thakɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ tibil na puno na pɛ war sora'.
54005008	Ado tibil na-n hɩɩn ɔɔ toa', dɩ ado aa-n hɩɩn ɔɔ cɔdara da-n jɔa', ha pɛrɛ a bo, a ka puurore a jɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ ha pɛdaara'.
54005009	Khikhɛrʋʋkɛ kanɩ yɛna kpalãther, ɔɔ i punone khere sɛbɛra, sɩ dɔ a do khɛrɩkɛ kɔɔ hɛnɩ kũu bɩɛl,
54005010	a dɔ khɛrɩkɛ hananɩ i bʋɔ thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛra, a dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ haanɛnɩ bɩsana, a dɔ dakha kpakpal tee khɛr, a dɔ ʋrɛ n kɔɔ tuonni da-n cʋʋ sikpulo thɔma tιι phuusɔra, na ʋrɛ n kɔɔ buloni wιrɛ n gaarɛnι, a dɔ dakha ʋrɛ n kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ thɔ̃ bɔ caar dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ.
54005011	Fa-n khere khikhɛraakɛ na tɩnanaa iə', gɩdonɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ thue n fʋ wɩnɩ gɩ-n cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wɩ hʋnɔna Kirisiti, dι wι-n ƴaalɛ ιnι-n birə hɛ kona,
54005012	dιι do wι hananɛ dιι gιrɛraakɛ wι phiini awι caca ʋlfɛɛkɛ wι kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanι Kirisiti.
54005013	Dɩ wo, wa hananɩ thɩ̃ɛ a na cʋa', wɩ-n ɩɩrɛ dɩ wa-n kpaar cɔna cɔna, sɩ gɩrɛ puuroni a jɔ dʋɔn mɔ̃ wɩ donɩ wɩrɛ n kpaarnanɩ sɔ, dɩ wa-n 'lɔɔ gɩrɛraakɛ na ba wɩna', dɩ wa-n mɩɩna thɩmɩaakɛ na teananɩ mɩɩra'.
54005014	Gɛr gɩ mɩ-n ƴaalɛ dɩ wɩrɛ na tɩnana' n birə hɛ kona, a hanana bɩsana, a jɩɛ fʋ awɩ cɔ, dɩ wa-n 'laa hʋɛ lãlaardaarra a na-n kʋɛ sɩ irə'.
54005015	Gɩdonɩ ɩkhasɔ kɔɔ 'lire kɛrrɛ gɩrɛ dɩ wa-n kpa Satana.
54005016	Ado ha pɛdaar hale, a kuun gɩ, a khɛr gɩ, a hana khikhɛra, ntɛsɔ na-n hɩnɛ wɩ, ga-n do we gbɛbɩdaraa heenda ga, dɩ mɛ̃ we gbɛbɩdara na puno na jɩɩ hɩɩn wɩrɛ jɩɛnnɩ do khikhɛra na sobɔr.
54005017	We gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔkɛ jɩɛnnɩ gba ƴɛ kʋʋlɛ wɩ teenanɛ cʋ dɛbɩnaa, sɩ wɩrɛ n gbũgbuloneni Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛra na tibil dɩɩrɛra, wɛr teana gɩ a jɔ.
54005018	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “Nakɩɩrɩkɛ na-n sanɩ jɔ, fa-n lii nʋɔa'.” Wo: “Thɔ̃daar teenanɛ ɔɔ lɩmɩ.”
54005019	Fa-n pɛ nũu sorιkɛ wa pɛnɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩna saagado gɩrɛ tɩbɩla yenyɔ dɩ yẽther gɩ tornɩ yirəə ga.
54005020	Wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ sopugo, phaanɛ wɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra, ga cʋʋrɛ dakha maar dι ga fʋ wɩrɛ sɛnɩ.
54005021	Mɩ-n kpãkpãa farɛ kheu Thãgbaa ƴɛra, na Jeju Kirisitii ƴɛra, na thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛ Thãgba phiirnii ƴɛra dɩ fa jɩɩ hɩɩn ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ, sɩ fa-n do tibil bo pɛrɛ na-n hale na dɩɩdɩɩ hɩɩna'.
54005022	Fa-n phana kɔrɔ a na dɛ̃ɛ tibillə nyɛ̃ɛ Thãgba thɔmana ga, dɩ fa-n do tibili sopugo n ma fa'. Jɩɛ fʋ dɩbara a 'lea dɩɩ.
54005023	Fa-n yɔ yɔ haar dɩbara bã, sɩ na 'lɛ taan gbegbe afɩ bɩ̃ khorara na afɩ tomɩraakɛra n sɛ fɩnɩ tɔ̃tɔ̃tɔ̃.
54005024	Ʋkhasɔ sopugo n yɩrrɛ sɩ dɩ kɩɩlʋ n pɩɩrɔ dɩɩ adã wɩ, sɩ ɩkhasɔɔda wer pɩpɩɩ paar gɩ-n yɩr.
54005025	Mɛna dakha thɔ̃ bʋɔ n yɩr, sɩ gɩrɛ na yɩrana' ga puno na too thale gɩ do gɩ kerra'.
54006001	Wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnι dea teenanɛ wa-n hɩnɛ awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ teenanɩ cʋʋr na sobɔr, dɩ mɛ̃ Thãgbaa i na kʋɛ dɩ dɩɩrɛɛkɛ sɩ-n dιιrnι ga.
54006002	Dι dee ƴιrɛ hananι kɔ̃tιna dι wι do ha pɛdara, wa-n 'lar õkũu dʋʋrra sι na beesi wa', sι wι ka na jιɛ do war thɔma gιdonι wιrɛ awɩ thɔ̃ɔle n bulni dɔ ha pɛdaraakɛ wɩ-n nanɩ. Na dɩrɛ ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ dɩ na kpãkpaanɛ gar.
54006003	Ado tibil na dɩɩr dɩɩr kpɩɩ, dɩ ado aa-n tu thɩmɩɩ bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitiida ga, na dɩɩrɛɛkɛ n jalanɩ kha na Thãgba fɩla',
54006004	ire ntɛ n ka mɔlɔ, aa jɩ thɩ̃a'; thɩ̃ bana tibil gɩ, na tɩɩ khɩɛsɩdaar, gɛr n ɩrɛna gbugi, na kɩla, na i kʋɛrɛ, na so jɩɩr na yinə,
54006005	na sɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃. Gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ har tɩbɩlalaakɛ fɩlɛ gõgolonɩ, wa-n mar dɩ wɩ jɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ sobɔr bã, dɩ wɩ-n kpɩɛrɛ Thãgba fɩl hananɛ dor lẽle thɩ̃ 'lɛ paar.
54006006	Sobɔr gɩ wer Thãgba fɩl hananɛ dor lẽle thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ tibillə ado a tu dɩ gɩrɛ ɩnɩ hananr dã nɛr mɛ̃.
54006007	Gιdonι sa kɔɔ hana thɩ̃ɛ a ιna kɛ thιɩra ga, dι a sa the sa puno a na gba thɩ̃ɛ dakha ga.
54006008	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ado sɩ hana dιkor na kẽkena, gele dã sɛr.
54006009	Sɩ wɩrɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩnɩ-n dɔ lẽledara, wɩ-n təəre ji fifiləlela, na pheruraakɛ dɔnι də̃bəəl thɩ̃ ƴaal jɔɔkɛ kpalanι ka, gɛr n hala tιbɩla dɩ wι mʋʋ kʋɛrɛra na bũburonena.
54006010	Gιdonι war naʋ dʋɔn sopugo jɔjʋɔɔ fʋ pa; dɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ ƴaalɛ gɩnɩ dɩ wa-n kpãkpaanɔ, wɩ faarɛ ha pɛrɛ sa gba dɩbara a mʋʋ ha hellela.
54006011	Sɩ fɛr Thãgbaa tibil, fe khiru pɛ ga thɩnaakɛ, sɩ na ƴaalɛ fɩl sarʋ, na Thãgba fɩlɛ, na ha pɛrɛ, na naʋ, na ha fʋrɛ, na hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ.
54006012	Na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ ha pɛ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ bʋɔ. Fɔrɔ yire khorr gɩrɛraakɛra Thãgba kɔɔ we fɩnɩ na gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ kɔɔ canɩ afι ha pɛ pasι tibil jɔjʋɔɔ ƴɛra.
54006013	Mɩ-n kpãkpãa farɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, ʋrɛɛkɛ n 'laanɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra yire, na Jeju Kirisitii ƴɛra, ʋrɛ kɔɔ cananι ɔɔ ha pɛ pasι Pɔ̃sι Pιlatιι ƴɛra,
54006014	dι fa jιι hιιn ga soolera ga hana sι paara', tibil na yιrɔ dakha dιa', phaphapha asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti n ɩna,
54006015	kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ̃ bɔɔ na danɩ dɩ Thãgba na nɩrɔ, Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ hɩnanɩ bɔnanɛ, ɔr bɩɛl dʋɔn Fãga hɩ̃daar, ɔr dʋɔn Fãgadaar kpɩɛ fãgadarara, na Kɔ̃tɩ̃ kpɩɛ kɔ̃tɩnana,
54006016	ɔr dɩbara na dɔ dakhinənə', ɔr haan dahɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ dadanana'; tibil bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ yɩa', dɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na puno na yɩa'. Ɔr teana a hɩna cʋrɛ na fãga khorr. Amɛn.
54006017	Kpãkpaanɛ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ lẽledarara wa-n ti gunə', wa-n gba awɩ nũ pɛ faa lẽle thɩɛnaakɛ na dɔ̃nɩ dapʋɔrnaa gaaga, sɩ wɩ faa Thãgbaraakɛ n 'laanɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛ̃ʋ dɩɩ dã sɩ thu, sɩ puno sɩ gba gɩ gɩ do asɩ kãkada.
54006018	Sɔ war wa-n cʋɛ bɔɔ, wɩ dɔ lẽledara thɔ̃ bɔ cnʋrɛra, wa-n 'laanɛ thɩ̃ɛ na haar, wa-n bulo tɩbɩla;
54006019	gɩ do mɛ̃ wɩ khɩɩ lẽle thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ dapʋɔrnaa a thɩɩn dɩɩ do bɔɔkɛ na ɩnanɩɩda, gɩ do yireekɛ wa 'lɛnɩ mɛ̃ gɩ jɩɩ do yi hana bɔ.
54006020	Timothe wei, jɩɛ fʋ gɩrɛ wɩ kɔɔ gbanɩ a dʋ fɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ. Golone folo folola na khaakhaar thɩmɩara, na thɩ̃ banaasɔraakɛ thɛnɩ jɩɩrraakɛ tɩbɩla n wenɩ jɩɩr sɩ ga do jɩɩr ga;
54006021	dɩ ɩkhasɔɔkɛ yɛnɩ ɩnɩ hana gɛr wɩ kɔɔ dɩrɛ hʋɛra, a lɛ̃, sa faa ha pɛrɛ. Thãgba na-n jɛ nɩ bʋɔra.
55001001	Mɛr Polɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirιsitii thɔ̃thɔn mɔ̃ Thãgba tuni dɩ ma-n mɩɩ yidaakɛ hanɩ Jeju Kirisitira, kɛ Thãgba yɩnɩ ɩna 'laarɛ,
55001002	mɛr thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Timotheekɛ dɔ marnɩ bikuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ: Thãgba Thιrɛ, na asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ fι bʋɔra a na-n dɔna fι dakha bʋɔ, a na-n hana fι dakha ha ιι.
55001003	Mι-n khιɩrɛ Thãgbaakɛ mɩ-n doronɩ thɔma ɩ̃ thɩthɩsɔɔ kha na kpɩɛrnɔ phuu; bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ-n jɩna fɩnɩ ɩ̃ Thãgba bɩɛlla dɩtɩnɛ na dɩwɩlʋ, mɩ-n khɩɩrɛ Thãgba.
55001004	A ma jɩna afɩ yilẽbi mɩ-n ƴaalɛ ka ɩ̃ yɛ fɩ daʋ n fʋ mɩ vʋ̃ʋ.
55001005	Mɩ-n jɩnanɛ dakha afɩ ha pɛɛkɛ na hananɩ fɩɩla'; dɩ afɩ nɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Lʋιsι na afι nι Enɩsɩ kɔɔ hana gɩ ɓo, dɩ mɩ jɩrɛ fι hana gɛr dakha.
55001006	Gɛr gι dɩ ma-n so far dι fa cʋʋ Thãgbaa khaardaakɛ fι kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ ɩ̃ nyɛ̃ dɛɛna ga-n jɩɩ le dɔ khaa.
55001007	Gɩdonɩ Thueekɛ Thãgba ha sɩnɩ na pɛ sar ha phaarɛ kpɩɩraka', sɩ fãga a na-n ha sɩ, na naʋ, na dɩbara fʋʋr.
55001008	Gɛr gɩ fa-n do yicuru na-n fʋ fɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩra ga, dɩ mɛrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ khaɩdaar ga, sɩ gaarɛ bʋɔ na mɛrɛ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra, gɩ the Thãgbaa fãgara.
55001009	Ɔr gɩɩkɛ kɔɔ taa sɩnɩ a we sɩ sɩ pho, sɩ ga do asɩ thɔ̃ cʋʋra gɩ tha', sɩ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ ƴaal hanɩ gɩ, na ɔɔ bɔ jɩɩkɛ a kɔɔ maanɩ thɩɩn sar kɛkɛkɛ dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the.
55001010	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ yɩranɩ nɛnɛ̃ Jeju Kirisiti asɩ Taadaarɩ ɩna, kɛ kɔɔ bũburoneni khir, sa gba tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ a nɩnana yireekɛ na dɔnɩ dapɩnana', dɩɩ yɩr dɩphã.
55001011	Ga tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra Thãgba pɛ mar dɩ ɩ̃ do ga mɩmɩɩ na thɔ̃thɔn na dɩɩrdaar.
55001012	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma-n gaar bʋɔ thakɛ sɩ yicuru na-n fʋ ma', gɩdonɩ mɩ jɩɛ jɩ ntɛɛkɛ mɩ pɛrnɩ haar, dɩ mι jɩrɛ tue gel dɩ a hananɛ punone a na hɩɩnna gɩrɛ a kɔɔ gbanɩ a dʋ mɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ gɩ dana ga Wiile.
55001013	Gba thɩmɩɩ bʋɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ ha fɩnɩ gɩ do far thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ fɩ jɩɩllɔ ha pɛrɛra, na naʋraakɛ sɩ hananɩ dɩɩ the asɩ bɩɛl dora na Jeju Kirisiti.
55001014	Thu Phuukɛ hanɩ asɩ bɩnɔ, jɩɛ fʋrɔ na ɔɔ fãga thɩ̃ bʋɔɔkɛ Thãgba dʋ fɩnɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
55001015	Fɩ jɩrɛ dɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ Ajɩ kɔɔ faa mɛr, ɩkhasɔ wɛrra dʋɔn Fɩjɛl na Ɛrmojɛn.
55001016	Kɔ̃tɩn n jɛ Onejɩfɔɔrɩ cɔdara wer bʋɔra, gɩdonι bɔ jɔjʋɔra ɔr n kɔɔ ƴɔla mɩ haar, dɩ yicuru na kɔɔ fʋʋ ɩ̃ khaιdaar dora ga;
55001017	sι ɔbɔɔkɛ a hanι Rɔm dιιra a ka kɔɔ ƴaal mɛr jɔɔ ka sa yι mι.
55001018	Kɔ̃tιn n jιɛnɛɛ bʋɔra ga Wirəəle gι the Kɔ̃tιnι pa. Fι jιrɛ bɔɔbɔɔ mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ bul mini jɔɔ Efɛjι dιιra.
55002001	Sι fɛr ɩ̃ bikuun, hanana fãga gι the bɔ jιιrraakɛ hanι Jeju Kirisitii pa.
55002002	Gιrɛ fι nιɛnι dι ɩ̃ mιιna tibil jɔjʋɔɔ ƴɛra, gba hana sobɔ tιbιlaakɛ na punoneni na dιιr dakha wɩ̃ tibil.
55002003	Gaarɛ bʋɔ nakha mɛrɛ a hɔ Jeju Kirisitii sɔrasι bɔ.
55002004	Tibil na ha sɔrasι cʋʋ paar sι a bir a faa ɔɔ kpιɛr nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ thιna, ado a-n ƴaalɛ a da ɔɔ sɔrasι kɔ̃tɩ̃ haara'.
55002005	Kɔlɔ̃kɔɔ can na 'li khor cacadaar dʋʋrra ado aa kɔɔ ca mɔ̃kɛ ga jɔfʋ sonaa ga.
55002006	Dɔ kokol n kɔɔ gbʋʋ yʋʋ kʋʋlɛla ɓo sɩ khar na-n kpaan.
55002007	Kpɩɛrɛ gɩrɛ mɩ sonɩ a hɩnɛ; Kɔ̃tɩn na hana fɩ kpɛsɛrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
55002008	Na jɛna Jeju Kirisitiikɛ dɔnɩ Davɩdɩɩ məl, ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ a the khirera mɔ̃kɛra tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ mɩ-n mɩɩnɩ sonɩ,
55002009	kɛ mɩ-n gaarɔnɩ bʋɔ gɩrɛ dɩ wɩ ba linə mi dɩ ɩ̃ ho puu cʋʋ tibil, sɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ wer na ha li paara'.
55002010	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ hana yɩrrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, wɩrɛ Thãgba phiirni n puno wɩ 'lɛ taarɛɛkɛ hanɩ Jeju Kirisitira na i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ khorrdaa.
55002011	Sobɔr thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ do gɩ yɩ: “Ado sɩ kɔɔ khire kha na ɔr, sa hananɛ kha dakha yire na ɔr.
55002012	Ado sa yɩr, sa bulle kha na ɔr ɔɔ fãgadaar dora. Ado sɩ bʋʋ, oti a na bo sɩ.
55002013	Ado sa do sobɔ tibilə', sobɔ tibillə or na dorakɛ 'lo, gɩdonɩ a na puno na debi ɔɔ fɩl dɩ ga ha kpɩɩ na gɩrɛ a dona'.”
55002014	Cʋɛ tɩbɩla wɩ jɩna ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ, dɩ na kpãkpaanɛ war kheu Thãgbaa ƴɛra wa-n bana mɔlɔ thɩ̃ banaa ga, ga do thɩ̃ bʋɔ ga, kʋɛrɛ gɩ-n do wɩrɛraakɛ n pɛ gɩnɩ nũu.
55002015	Gbuoro yʋʋ na jɩlɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra mɔ̃ fɩ donɩ thɔ̃daarɩkɛ daaraanɩ haar sɩ yicuru na fʋ fa', sɩ fɩ do ʋrɛ n 'laanɛnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ dẽdẽdẽ.
55002016	Golone folo folola na khaakhaar thɩmɩara, gɩdonɩ wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ ga thɩ̃ɩle gɩ-n cʋʋ wɛr dɩ awɩ Thãgba fɩl 'lee n puuro dɩ ga-n pɛr.
55002017	Awɩ thɩmɩɩ dakha n ƴɛrrɛ nɔr khaa, mɛ̃ gɩ ha na Imene na Fɩlɛtɩ,
55002018	kɛ kɔɔ dɛnɩ hʋɛra a lɛ̃ sa faa sobɔr dɩ wa-n mɩɩ ayɩ: Khi ɩɩrɛ mãa kpãsɛrɛ; dɩ wɩ cʋʋrɛ ɩkhasɔɔ ha pɛ dɩɩ kʋɛ.
55002019	Sɩrakɛ Thãgbaa gookɛ a kpɛɛnɩ gɩ jɩɩlɛ kɩbɩ, a hana thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ dɔnɩ jɩɩn dɩɩ so ayɩ: “Kɔ̃tɩn jɩrɛ wɩrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔda.” Wo: “Tibil wo tibilikɛ yɛnɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda ɩnɩ do, dɔ a hʋnɔna sopugo.”
55002020	Cɔ kɔ̃tɩɩna, ga-n do bʋlaakɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ dɛ na gɩrɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ dɛ bulona n haanle dɩbara ga, sɩ thɩrdaa n hale dakha na jadaa, dɩ yɛ n dor bʋla ɓʋ̃ɔ sɩ yɛ n do thɔ̃ pɔɩ cʋʋdaa.
55002021	Dɩ ado tibil fʋ dɩbara a phu ga sopugosɔraale, ɔr na dɔ bʋla ɓʋ̃ɔ, kɛ Thãgba thɩɩnnɩ kpɩɩ, dɩɩ do bɔ taa thɩ̃ɛ Kɔ̃tɩnna, a too ga too a na-n do thɔ̃ bɔ caar dɩɩdɩɩ fɛʋ.
55002022	Gɩrɛ n kɔnɩ daɓola thue, fe khiru pɛ gar, sɩ na ƴaalɛ fɩl sarʋ, na ha pɛrɛ, na naʋ, na ha ɩɩ, nakha wɩrɛɛkɛ n fʋɔrɛnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn na ha phuu.
55002023	Bɔ də̃bəəl thɩ̃ bananɛɛkɛ na hananɩ kɩrʋa', gɩdonɩ fɩ jɩrɛ gɛr n ɩrɛna kɩla.
55002024	Dɩ ga teena Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɔ̃daar na-n ɩrɛna kɩla ga, a ka teenanɛ a hanana hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ na tɩbɩla fɛʋ, a dɔ dakha tibilikɛ n punoneni da-n dɩɩr tibil thɩ̃ɛ; a dɔ ha fʋ tibil,
55002025	a hanana ha bulole mɔ̃ a-n narnɩ wɩrɛ na-n tuonni dɩɩra', a na pɛna nũu mɔ̃ ga donɩ Thãgba cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wɩ debi haar a jɩ gɩrɛ n dɔnɩ sobɔr,
55002026	gɩ cʋʋ dakha kpɩɛrɛ gɩ lõ war wɩ taa Satãa pherra, kɛ fɔ wɩnɩ ɩɩrɔ wa-n cʋɛ ɔɔ tuur.
55003001	Jɛna dɩ pɩpɩɩ wiresɔra bɔ puu na hale.
55003002	Gɩdonɩ tɩbɩla na dor dɩbara nadara, war nadara, nɔfa mɩɩdara, i yaaldara, Thãgbaa i kʋɛdara, thɛ na nɛɛ nũ nʋʋrdara, wa jɩ fɛr hɩna fʋɔra', wa dor Thãgba bodara,
55003003	wa hana pərrə', wa dor nɔ ɓaar tɩbɩla, tibil i kʋɛdara, dɩbara fʋ 'leedara, ha khedara, fɩl bɔ bodara,
55003004	tibil liirdara, wolo wolodara, i kadara, gɩrɛ n kɔnɩ tibil thuee ƴaal na har awɩ hara a na jɔ Thãgba ƴaalɛ;
55003005	sɩrakɛ wɩ hor Thãgba fʋɔrdara sɩɩ do wɩ bor ga fãgaale. Hʋnɔnɛna wa tibil casɔɔle.
55003006	Wɛ n hale awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn dɩ wɩ wolõ a lõ tɩbɩlaa cɔ a fʋlɛ khɛr surosɔɔkɛ sopugo doronɩ dɛr a ɩɩrɔ, kɛ dɔnɩ khɛ ƴɩrɛ thɩ̃ caar dɩɩdɩɩ n kʋnɩ thue ka,
55003007	kɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ wa-n dɩɩr thɩ̃ɛ wire koo, sι wa-n mar kpɩɩrakɛ a na dã a na jɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ sobɔra'.
55003008	Mɔ̃kɛ Janɛsɩ na Jãbɩrɛsɩ kɔɔ bãbaranɩ Mʋɩjɩ, mɛna wa tibil casɔɔle n bãbarã sobɔr. Tɩbɩla wɛɛkɛ awɩ kpɩɛr na telena', dɩ wa do bɔ taa tɩbɩla ha pɛdaara ga.
55003009	Dɩ wa puno na jal ƴɔɔ bã, gɩdonɩ awɩ də̃bəəl na yɩrrɛ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ mɔ̃kɛ kona yenyɔɔleeda kɔɔ yɩrnɩ.
55003010	Sɩ fe wer, fɩ kpaanɛ ɩ̃ dɩɩrra dɔdɔdɔ, na ɩ̃ cʋʋ para, na gɩrɛ mɩ jɩɩllɔnɩ, na ɩ̃ ha pɛra, na ɩ̃ ha fʋra, na ɩ̃ naʋra, na ɩ̃ yʋ gbuurə,
55003011	na ɩ̃ kpoora, na ɩ̃ bɔ gaarra. Fɩ jɩrɛ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ dana mɩnɩ Ãtɩyɔsɩ, na Ɩkɔn, na Lisitiri, kpoore mɩ kɔɔ yɩ gɩmɔ̃, sɩ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ taa mɛr gelela fɛʋ.
55003012	Dɩrakɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ ɩna-n ɩrɛ na Thãgba fɩlɛ awɩ bɩɛl dora na Jeju Kirisiti, wa yɩrɛ kpoore.
55003013	Sɩ tɩɩ puusɔ na tɩɩ fɩɩldara wa puurore wa-n pɛr, wa dor tɩɩ fɩɩldara wɩ dona dakha wɩrɛ n fɩlɛnɩ dɩbara.
55003014	Sɩ fɛrɛ, jɩɛ jɩɩl gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ kɔɔ dɩɩrnɩ, kɛ fɩ jɩnɩ tue dɩɩ do gɛr dɔ sobɔr, gɩdonɩ fɩ jɩrɛ dakha tibil ʋrɛ kɔɔ dɩrɛ fɩnɩ.
55003015	Dɩ a fʋna afɩ bɩsã bu bɔɔ, fɩ jɩrɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ phu, gɛr na punone na ha fɩ kpɛsɛrɛ taa 'lɛrraakɛ fa 'lɛnɩ gɩ the ha pɛrɛraakɛ fa hananɩ Jeju Kirisitira.
55003016	Thãgbaa sɛbɛɛ thɩmɩɩ fɛʋ dɔ gɩrɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa nɔɔ, dɩ gɩ dor dabʋɔ ka a na dɩɩr tibil thɩ̃ɛ, a na nɩna tibil dι paar, a na naar tibil, a na dιιr tibil a na pɛ dateleena,
55003017	gι do nɔɔ Thãgbaa tibil n 'li dιbara, a gbɛbι a ma thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛra fɛʋ.
55004001	Mɩ-n kpãkpãa farɛ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra na Jeju Kirisitii ƴɛra, na mɔ̃ gɩ donɩ Kirisitira na bire na ɩ̃ a na kɩɩlna yidara na khe, saa gba ɔɔ fãga, mɩ so farɛ gɩrɛ ayɩ:
55004002	Na mɩa Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ, na yɩrana gɩ, a fɩ yɩrɛ fʋ paar a fa yɩ fʋ paara'; na nɛna tɩbɩla awɩ dɩ pa, na naarɛ wɩ, na kpãkpaanɛ war, sɩ na cʋɛ gele na ha fʋrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɩɩrdaar teenanɩ a hanana.
55004003	Gɩdonɩ bɔ bɩɛl na daan kɛ tɩbɩla na tuni dɩɩr bʋɔ bã, sɩ mɔ̃kɛ awɩ bɩ̃ n nanɩ dɩ awɩ nũ na-n hʋʋl wɩ thɩ̃ kpɩɩ nɩɩrra, wa ƴaalɛ dɩɩrdara wa-n ɓã dɩɩrdarara.
55004004	Wa kpʋʋ garɛ nũu sobɔ nɩɩrra, sɩ wa-n pɛ kpuro nɩɛsɔ nũu.
55004005	Sɩ fe wer, a gɩ ha mɔ̃ na fɔ haar, fa-n hə̃jə̃ə bɔ gaarɛra ga, dɔ thɔ̃ don tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛra, na dɔ afɩ thɔ̃ ga-n pɩ ɓibi.
55004006	Gɩdonɩ ado me wer gɩ, bɔɔ daan dɩ ɩ̃ tɔmɩ̃ na deer, ɩ̃ kɔ̃ bɔ wɔrɔnɛ dɩphã.
55004007	Mɩ kɔɔ kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ bʋɔ; mɩ car ɩ̃ kɔlɔ̃kɔɔ pɩ, mɩ fʋrɛ ha pɛrɛ kĩkĩ.
55004008	Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã khorɩkɛ ma 'lɛnɩ cacadaar dʋʋrra n pɩɛrɛ mɩ mɛ̃, gɛr dʋɔn so hɛl khaardaakɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ n kɩlɛnɩ kɩɩl telẽe na ha mɩnɩ ga Wirəəle, sɩ ga do mɛr dɩbara a na ha ga, sɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n naannɩ ɔɔ bir ɩ̃.
55004009	Dɔ bʋɔ sa ɩna ɩ̃ pa kɔrɔ,
55004010	gɩdonɩ Demasɩ faa mɛr dɩ gɩ ther naʋraakɛ a-n nanɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛɛ thɩna, Tesalonɩkɩ a jal, dɩ Kiresã jal Galasɩ, Tɩtɩ jal Dalmasɩ;
55004011	Luki dɩbara haan kha na mɛrɛ; kpa Markɩ nɩ ɩ̃ kha gɩdonɩ a do marɛ bɔ taa tibil thɔmana.
55004012	Tɩsɩkɩ wer mɛr thɔnaa Efɛjɩ.
55004013	A fa ɩ̃ gba ɩ̃ delkeba jakparaakɛ mɩ faanɩ Tʋrʋasι Karpusii pa, a gbana dakha sɛbɛsɔ, sι caca thɩ̃ɛ dʋɔn ɩ̃ lo sɛbɛ.
55004014	Phube Alesãdɩɩr kɔɔ cʋʋ mɛr puure ka; Kɔ̃tɩn na lɩmaa mɔna ɔɔ thɔna hanɩ.
55004015	Fɛrɛ dakha na jɩɛ dʋʋraa bʋrɛ dɛ, gɩdonɩ a bana mɛr waa gel ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩsɔraakɛ mɩ kɔɔ mɩɩnɩ.
55004016	Caca bɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ jɩɩlnɩ ɩ̃ hɛl ɩ̃ so, tibil bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ jɩɩl mara', sɩ fɛʋ kɔɔ faa mɛr. Thãgba na-n gba gele wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ a heen wa'.
55004017	Kɔ̃tɩn dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ jɩlɛna mɩnɩ a ha mɩ fãga dɩɩ do nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ mɩɩ tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ waa dιɩ dã thu, dɩ ca kpala fɛʋ nɩɛ. Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ taa mɩ sidũ'ũ gbuokhorə.
55004018	Kɔ̃tɩnna na-n taa mɩ thɔ̃ puu caarra fɛʋ, dɩ a na fʋ marɛ na cʋʋ mɩ dɩ ma lõ ɔɔ ƴũ fãga dιra. Ɔɔ i n dʋbarɔ na jala waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
55004019	Fʋɔrɛ Pirisika na Akɩlasɩ na Onejɩfɔɔrɩ cɔdara.
55004020	Erasɩtɩ wer toore Korɛ̃tɩ, sɩ gɩ-n khor Tʋrofɩm dɩ ɩ̃ sɩɩraa dɩ too Mɩle.
55004021	Bãbanɛ a dana kɛ sɩ yʋʋr n yo. Ebulusi, Pudãsɩ, Linusi, Kʋlodιa na omɩna fɛʋ wɩ fʋɔr fɛr.
55004022	Kɔ̃tɩn n hana kha na fɛrɛ. Thãgba na-n jɛ nɩ bʋɔra.
56001001	Mɛr Polιkɛ dɔnι Thãgbaa thɔ̃daar na Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn, gι cʋʋ wιrɛ Thãgba phiirni wι 'lɛ ha pɛrɛ, wι 'lɛna dakha sobɔ jιιrιkɛ n cʋranι kha na Thãgba fιlɛ,
56001002	wa-n pɛna nũu yire khorrιkɛ Thãgbaakɛ na-n sõsonena' kɔɔ maanι ʋlfɛrɛ kɛkɛkɛ ιna 'laarɛ,
56001003	dι ɔbɔɔkɛ bɔɔkɛ a pɛrnι danι, a kɔɔ nιnanɛ ɔɔ thιmιιkɛra ɔr Thãgba asι Taadaar yιnι ma-n mιa;
56001004	mι thɔnanɛ sɛbɛɛkɛ ɩ̃ ha fɛr Tιtɩɩkɛ dɔ marnι bikuun ha pɛrɛraakɛ sι bulni kha. Thãgba Thιrɛ, na Jeju Kirisiti asι Taadaar na-n jɛ nι bʋɔra, a na-n hana nι dakha ha ιι.
56001005	Mι kɔɔ faa fɛr Kιrɛtι fι gbɛbι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ sɛnι gɩ telẽ, dɩ fɔ mɔ̃ mɩ kɔɔ so farnɩ sa pɩɛr we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ dɩɩdɩɩsɔra;
56001006	sɩ dɔ ntɛ n do kuunikɛ na hananɩ so paara', a hanana khɛ bɩɛl, a hanana bɩsanaakɛ dɔnɩ ha pɛdara, kɛ tɩbɩla na pɛrnɩ sor dakhaba dʋʋrra dɩ nũ nʋʋrɛra ga.
56001007	Gɩdonɩ we gbɛbɩdaarɩ hɩɩndaar teenanɛ a dɔ ʋrɛ na hananɩ so paar mɔ̃ a donɩ Thãgbaa thɩ̃ hɩɩndaara', a na-n do tibilikɛ na-n wuronəə ga, a na-n gba nĩkhii kɔrɔa', a na-n do ta laardaar na kιl ƴaal tibilə', a na-n phʋʋn tιbɩla na fãga bɩɩ ɔɔ war ƴaalla ga,
56001008	sɩ a dɔ kpakpal tee tibil, a dɔ tibilikɛ n naannɩ gɩrɛ telenenɩ, a dɔ yʋ bɔ tibil, a dɔ tɩɩ sarʋ, a hanana fɩl phuu, a dɔ dɩbara fʋdaar.
56001009	A teenanɛ a jɩɛ ma bɔɔbɔɔ sobɔ thɩmɩɩrraakɛ n thɛnɩ dɩɩrɛra, dɩ mɛ̃ a na mar a gba dɩɩr bʋɔ a na-n dɩɩr tibil, a na-n punona dakha thɩ̃ banadara.
56001010	Gɩdonɩ jɔɔ hale khʋ̃ kurdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn, kɛ na-n tuonni thɩmɩɩra', kɛ dɔnɩ mɔlɔ thɩ̃ banadara na tɩɩ fɩɩldara,
56001011	kɛ teananɩ sɩ khaanɛ wɩ nʋɔ; a wɩ lõ cɔ dɔɔra wɩ-n nyanyãa gɛr koo, wɩ-n dɩɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na teananɩ dɩɩra' wɩ puno wa-n 'lɛ yicur war.
56001012	Awɩ thɛthɛɛ bobon bɩɛl yɛrɛrakɛ sor ayɩ: “Kɩrɛtɩdara wer, sɔ̃sɔ wɩ-n kuur wire fɛʋ, hɔ̃ nʋ̃ puunə ha wɩ, khãkhalaakɛ n kɛbanɩ wɩ do.”
56001013	Dɩ sobɔrra gɩ do ger; gɛr gɩ phaanɛ wɩ dakɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ wɩ jɩɛ hana ha pɛ bʋɔ,
56001014	dɩ wa-n bo na pɛ nũu Juifisɔɔ kpuro nɩra ga, dɩ jɔfʋraakɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ faanɩ sobɔr pɛrnɩ ga.
56001015	Thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ phure wɩrɛraakɛ phonɩ, sɩ thɩ̃ bɩɛllakɛ na phu wɩrɛraakɛ bisenenə', kɛ dɔnɩ ha pɛ 'leedara ga; awɩ fɩl na awɩ kpɩɛrnɔ bisere.
56001016	Sɩ nʋɔ wer n mɩɩrɛ ɩnɩ jɩrɛ Thãgba, sɩ awɩ cʋʋ pa na-n jal kha na gιrɛ wι-n sona'. Tιι sʋ̃ɔ ha wι na nũ nʋra, wa-n puno thɩ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛ fιιʋraka'.
56002001	Sɩ ado fɛr gɩ, na dɩrɛ ga-n jal mɔ̃kɛ dɩɩr bʋɔ hanɩ.
56002002	Sɔ kũu kɔ̃tɩnana dɩ wa hana dɩbara fʋrɛ, wɩ dɔ dakha tɩɩ cʋnanɛ, a dɔna yʋ bɔ tɩbɩla, wɩ tɛ ha pɛrɛra, na naʋra, na ha fʋrɛra.
56002003	Sɔ dakha khɛ kpɛɛnana wɩ dɔ awɩ cʋʋ pa na-n nɩna gɩrɛ n dɔnɩ phur; wa-n do i kʋɛ khɛra ga, wa-n do taanɩ dea', sɩ wɩ dɔ khɛraakɛ hananɩ dɩɩr bʋɔ,
56002004	dɩ mɛ̃ wa puno a na dɩɩr khɛ bɩsana wa-n na awɩ ko, nakha awɩ bɩsãsɔ,
56002005	wɩ do dakha khɛraakɛ hanɩ hɛlɛlɛ, wɩ hanana fɩl phuu, wɩ dona dakha wɩrɛ n jɩɛnnɩ do awɩ cɔka thɔ̃, wɩ dona dakha khɛraakɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ, wɩ jo dakha awɩ kora gɩ do nɔɔ tibil na puno na kpɛ Thãgbaa soa'.
56002006	Sɔ daɓolala dakha dɩ wa fʋ dɩbara;
56002007	sɩ fɛrɛ dakha fɩ do thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛra mɔ̃ fɩ-n dɩɩrnɩ tɩbɩla na fɩl bʋɔ na cʋ hananɛ,
56002008	ga-n dɔ thɩmɩɩ bʋɔɔkɛ tibil na yɩnɩ kpɛ paara', dɩ mɛ̃ yicuru na fʋ asɩ lãlaardaar a na yɩ asɩ dapuu mɩɩ pa ga.
56002009	Sɔ deara dɩ wa jo dɩbara awɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔra, a na da war haar thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, wa-n bana wɩ thɩ̃ banaa ga,
56002010	wa-n yu thɩ̃a', sɩ wa-n nɛna wɩ wire fɛʋ awɩ sobɔdaar do, gɩ do thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩɛna gɩ cʋʋrɛ Thãgba asɩ Taadaarɩ dɩɩr dɩ ga hana cʋrɛ.
56002011	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ taa 'lɛ pa gɩ yɩrrɛ dɩphã;
56002012	gɩ-n dɩɩr sɛr dɩ sa faa thɩ̃ gõgolõ na thɩɩkɛɛ ha pɩɛr, sɩ sɩ too nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔraakɛra sɩ hana dɩbara fʋrɛ, na fɩl telẽe, na Thãgba fɩlɛ,
56002013	sa-n pɩɛrna kãka wireekɛ sa tornɩ yire gɩrɛra sɩ-n kɔɔ pɛnɩ nũu, kɛ dɔnɩ mɔ̃ asɩ Thãgba Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na Taadaar Jeju Kirisiti na-n ɩnɩ na i dʋbɩrɛ.
56002014	Ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ faanɩ ɔɔbara asɩ sora, dɩ mɛ̃ a birse si a ti si sopugosɔra fɛʋ, sa phʋɔl sɩ sɩ dɔ caarɩkɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛda, kɛ thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛ n kʋnɩ thue.
56002015	Na mɩa ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ, na kpãkpaanɛ tɩbɩlala, na nɛna wɩ awɩ dɩ pa, gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩn ha fɛr hʋɛ. Fa-n do tibil na-n beesi fa'.
56003001	Na khɛ war wa-n jɔ dɩbara fãgadarasɔra na kɔ̃tmasɔra, wa-n nɛ nũu, wɩ tɔɔ thɔ̃ bʋɔ fɛʋʋ cʋʋ too,
56003002	wa-n mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ puu tibillə ga, sɩ wɩ dɔ ha ie ƴaal tɩbɩla, na bɩ̃ bɔ tɩbɩla, na hɛlɛlɛ fɩldara tɩbιlala fɛʋ.
56003003	Gιdonι sɛrɛ dakha thalera sι kɔɔ ha, sι kɔɔ dor də̃bələ, na nũ nʋra, sι kɔɔ buure, a dona dakha ha pιɛr dea thɩ̃ɛsɔraakɛ n kɔ sɩnɩ thue; sι kɔɔ hananɛ bɩ̃ puu na gbugi, dι sι kɔɔ teenanɛ laarɛ dι dakha sι-n laarɛ khasɔ.
56003004	Sι ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι asι Taadaarι ha bulo fιl na ɔɔ naʋ tιbιlala yιrnι,
56003005	gɛr a kɔɔ taa sar, sι ga do fιl sar thɔ̃ dιkha sι kɔɔ cʋa', sι ɔɔ bɔ jιra gι, mɔ̃ a cɔcɔɔ sιnι a cʋʋ sɩ dι sι kɔ̃ daphaa, kɛ dɔnι tibil pha dʋʋrιkɛ Thu Phuu cʋʋ sιnι dι sι do;
56003006	dι Jeju Kirisiti asι Taadaar dɔ nɔɔ dι sι 'lɛ Thu Phuulera dιι və̃vĩə,
56003007	gι do nɔɔ gιdonι sor hɛl sarɛ bɔ jιιrra pι, sι debi sι do wιrɛ na 'lɛnι yire khorrιkɛra sι-n pɛnι nũu.
56003008	Sobɔr thιmιιrιkɛ do, dι mι-n ƴaalɛ fι bɔ na ιa gar, dι mɛ̃ wιrɛ pιɛrnι haar Thãgbara na gbuuro yʋʋ wa-n cʋʋ thɔ̃ bʋɔ; gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ telenenι a bɔr tιbιlala dι wa cʋʋ.
56003009	Sɩ golone də̃bəəl thɩ̃ bana bananɛna, na thɩ kɔ̃ jɔfʋ thɩmɩɩrra, na kɩlasɔ, na thɩ̃ banaa jɔfʋdaara, gɩdonɩ ga do bɔ taa thɩ̃ɛ ha gela', mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ gɩ.
56003010	A fɩ kpãkpãa ʋrɛraakɛ n pɩɛrnɩ leere dɩɩ dã babɩɛl na balanyɔ dɔrɔɔm, fa-n do nɩ ha kha dɩkha bã.
56003011	Jɛna dɩ tibil ca ole kʋɛrɛ koo, sopugo a-n cʋʋ da-n heen sor dɩbara.
56003012	Ɔbɔɔkɛ ma thɔ̃ farnɩ Artemasɩ agɩbo Tɩsɩkɩ bãbanɛ sa caanɛ mɩ Nɩkopolɩsɩ, gɩdonɩ mɩ kpɩɛrɛ sa yɩ le ma too yʋʋrɔ.
56003013	Gʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ Jenasɩ jɔfʋ dɩɩrdaar na Apolɔsɩɩ kpaarda a pɛ wɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛ na ɓɔr wa'.
56003014	Dɔ asɩ too dakha n dɩɩr wa-n do thɔ̃ bʋɔ wɩ puno wa-n bul wɩrɛ gɩ-n ɓɔrnɩ ɓɔr bʋɔ, wa-n too gɩ do ga do bɔ taa tɩbɩla ha waa ga.
56003015	Wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ kha na mɛrɛ wɩ fʋɔr fɛr. Fʋɔrɛ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n naan sɩnɩ, kɛ sɩ donanɩ kha ha pɛdara. Thãgba na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra.
57001001	Mɛr Polιkɛ dɔnι khaιdaar Jeju Kirisitii sora, na asι omi Timothe, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha fɛr Filemɔ̃ɔkɛ sι-n nanι, kɛ sι-n donanι kha thɔma,
57001002	a hana dakha asι õkhɛr Afιa na Arsιpιιkɛ sι-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnanι kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ bιɛl, na we gbɛbιdaraakɛ n gbɛbanι kha afι cɔ.
57001003	Thãgba asι Thι na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tιn na-n jɛ nι bʋɔra a na hana nι dakha ha ιι.
57001004	Wire fɛʋ mι-n khιι ɩ̃ Thãgba dι ma-n bιɛlna dι ma-n pɛ far,
57001005	gιdonι mι nιɛrɛ mɔ̃ afι naʋʋkɛ fι hananɩ Jeju Kɔ̃tɩnna na tɩɩ phuusɔra fɛʋ hanɩ, na mɔ̃ afɩ ha pɛ hanɩ.
57001006	Mɩ-n bɩɛlɛ Thãgba dɩ afɩ ha pɛ hana n dɔ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hananɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ gι do Kirisitiida dɔ nɔɔ, gι cʋʋ tιbιla wa-n yι sar thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋ caar dɩɩdɩɩ.
57001007	Daʋ fʋ mɛr jɔɔ ka dɩ afɩ naʋ dor nɔɔ dɩ ɩ̃ faa haar; gɩdonɩ fɛr dɔ nɔɔ, ɩ̃ omi, dɩ mãthɩ̃ɩ na-n the tɩɩ phuusɔɔ nɔɔ.
57001008	Kirisiti ha mɛr hʋɛ gbobi dɩ ma puno na so far nayɩ: Fɩ teenanɛ;
57001009	sɩ naʋ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ ma-n phʋʋr fɩ, mɛr Polɩkɛ dɔnɩ kũu kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, a dona dakha nɛnɛ̃ khaɩdaar Jeju Kirisitii sora.
57001010	Mɩ-n phʋʋr fɛr ɩ̃ bɩsã Onejɩmɩdara, kɛ debanɩ a do ɩ̃ bikuun bɔɔraakɛ mɩ hanɩ khaɩra,
57001011	kɛ mamara na kɔɔ dɔ farnɩ bɔ taa tibilə', sɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔ taa tibil a do, sɩ ga do fɛrɛra dɩbara ga, sɩ na mɛrɛra dakha.
57001012	Mɩ bire thɔnaa ma-n ha fɩ sɩ ɩ̃ yi bi a do.
57001013	Mɩ kɔɔ ƴaalɛla dɩ na toona mɩ a na-n do mɩ thɔmaakɛ fa kɔɔ do mɩnɩ bɔɔraakɛ mɩ hanɩ khaɩra tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩra.
57001014	Sɩ ma ƴaal ɩ̃ cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ sɩ ga do fɛr hana mɩ hʋɛa ga, dɩ mɛ̃ ga-n do afɩ bɔ cʋʋ dor fɛrɛ pɛra', sɩ gɩ do afɩ ƴaalla gɩ the.
57001015	Anaa gɛr a kɔɔ faa far bɔɔ gbe, sɩ fɩ bir fɩ 'lɩɛ waa khorr;
57001016	sɩ ga do dee khaa bã, sɩ a ba dee, omineekɛ fa-n nanɩ a na do. Mɩ naarɛ ka, sɩ fɛr na naanɛɛnakɛ na ka na jɔ, mɔna a donɩ dee na Kɔ̃tɩnɩda.
57001017	Dɩ gɛr gɩ ado fɩ-n hɩɩn mɛr dɩ ɩ̃ do afɩ kuun, teaa mɔ̃ fa tee mɩnɩ.
57001018	Dɩ ado a cʋʋ fɛr puu dɔɔ mɔnakɛ, dɩ a helu gɩ dɩ hana fɩ, dɔ gɩ ha ɩ̃ yʋɔ.
57001019	Mɛr Pol khera gɩrɛ na ɩ̃ thɛthɛɛ nyɛ̃ ayɩ: Mɛr na lɩma fɛʋ. Sɩ ma so far nayɩ, yireekɛ fɩ hananɩ helu gɩ dι fι hana ma'.
57001020	Mɛ̃ gι ɩ̃ omi, cʋɛ mι bɔ ca ʋrɛ gι do Kɔ̃tιn dɔ nɔɔ; cʋɛ mãthɩ̃ι n the mι nɔɔ Kirisitiida dʋʋrra.
57001021	Mɔ̃ mι jιnι dι fa pɛ mɛr nũu mι khere farɛ sɛbɛɛkɛ, mι jιrɛrakɛ dι fa cʋʋrɛ dι ga jɔ gιrɛɛkɛ mι sonι.
57001022	Sι wo, gbɛbιrɛ mar cɔ paar gιdonι mι pɛrɛ haar anι Thãgba bιɛlla na dor nɔɔ dι wa faa mι.
57001023	Epafιrasιιkɛ sι hananι kha khaιra dιι do Jeju Kirisitiida dɔ nɔɔ, a fʋɔr fɛr.
57001024	Wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ sι-n donanι kha thɔma, Markι na Arιsιtarkι na Demasι na Luki, wι fʋɔr fɛr dakha.
57001025	Asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra.
58001001	Mamara Thãgbaa bobonaa nɔ Thãgba kɔɔ gba bɔɔ dɩɩdɩɩra na thɩmɩɩ ƴιɛ dɩɩdɩɩ a mɩɩna asɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ,
58001002	sɩ pɩpɩɩ bɔɔraakɛ Bikuun a gba a mɩɩna sɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ a pɛrnɩ dɩ do thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ hɩ̃hɩ̃, ɔrra dakha a gba a tinə thɩɩ na ƴũ.
58001003	Ɔɔ pa Thãgbaa i dʋbɩɩkɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ n yɩr; ɔɔ pa tibil na yɩ gbelẽ gbelẽ mɔ̃ Thãgba dʋʋr hanι; ɔɔ nɔ thιmιιkɛ hananι fãga ka a fʋna thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dιι jιιl. Ɔr kɔɔ cʋɛ sopugo hɛl thɔma sa too gιrɛ Thãgba dawabʋʋ nyɔ̃bɔra le ƴũ pər.
58001004	Mɛ̃ Bikuun kɔ̃tɩ̃ a jɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ fĩi, mɔ̃ a 'lɛnι ireekɛ kɔ̃tιnanι dιι jɔ awιda.
58001005	Gιdonι ʋmɔ̃ɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu Thãgba kɔɔ sor ayι: “Fɛr dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuun, mɛr Thãgba kɔna fɩ nĩ gɩrɛ.” Wo: “Ma dʋʋraarɛ Thɩrɛ a do mar Bikuun.”
58001006	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a birni thɔ̃ ɔɔ caca Bikuun thɩɩraakɛ a sor ayɩ: “Dɔ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ fɛʋ n gburõku wa-n fʋɔrʋʋ.”
58001007	Sι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔdara wer a sor ayι: “A-n cʋʋrɛ ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ dι wι do jɩɛ, dɩ cʋʋ dakha ɔɔ thɔ̃dara dι wι do dɔlιnanɛ.”
58001008	Sι Bikuunida wer a sor ayι: “Afι fãga too pa ya Thãgba, khorrdaa gɩ waa vʋ̃ʋ. Afɩ fãgadaar do, fɩl sar fãgadaar dʋʋr gɩ.
58001009	Fɩ nar fɩl sarʋ sa laar fιl gõgolõ, gɛr gι Thãgbaakɛ dɔnι afι Thãgba phiir fi, mɔ̃ a bʋl fιnι niin, kɛ dɔnι da niin, dι fι jɔr gιrɛ afι kuunsɔ fɛʋ.”
58001010	Wo: “Fɛr Kɔ̃tɩn, kɛkɛkɛra fɛr kɔɔ te thɩɩ, dɩ thãgbara ƴũ dɔ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ fɩ cʋʋnɩ na afɩ nyɛ̃.
58001011	Gelesɔ ga kʋɛrɛ, sɩ fe wer fɩ toonɩ fɩ toore, ga tɩnɛsɔ fɛʋ kẽkẽ khaa.
58001012	Fa pur gersɔ kʋla kʋla dɛbɛ khaa, dɩ ga debire kẽkẽ khaa. Sɩ fe wer ɔmɛna fer toorakɛ a ha, afɩ yɛ na hana ga pɩra'.”
58001013	Dɩ ʋmɔ̃ɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu Thãgba kɔɔ sor ayɩ: “Tɔɔ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra phaphapha ɩ̃ cʋʋ afι lãlaardara wι do afι nɛ jəəda.”
58001014	Ga do thuesɔ wι do fɛʋ a ha Thãgbaa thɔna, dι thɔ̃ wι wa-n bulo wιrɛ teananι wι 'lɛ taaraa?
58002001	Gɛr dɔ kιrʋ gι teenanɛ sa-n bãbanɛ a jιɛ mar yʋʋ gιrɛraakɛ sι kɔɔ nιɛnι, a ga ha mã', sa tɔr na khokhιa gar.
58002002	Gιdonι ado thιmιιrιkɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ kɔɔ mιιnι gι kɔɔ nιnanɛ dι sobɔr gι do, dι ado jɔfʋ kʋɛrɛ fɛʋ na nũ nʋʋrɛ fɛʋ kɔɔ 'lɛr sor dιι tee kha,
58002003	sɛrɛ mɔ̃ sa fuu ado sa-n pər taarɛraakɛ kɔ̃tιnanι thaka? Kɛ dɔnι gιrɛ Kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ ιιrnanι a mιι, dι wιrɛ kɔɔ nιɛnɛnι bir gba a mιι sι dι sobɔr gι do.
58002004	Thãgba kɔɔ gbaar jιιnsɔ, na ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛsɔ, na nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ dιιdιι, na Thu Phuu khaardasɔɔkɛ a-n tιnɛnι mɔ̃ a-n ƴaalnι, a gba gɛr a nιnana dι gιrɛra wι-n mιιnι sobɔr gι.
58002005	Gιdonι ga do thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔra Thãgba kɔɔ jo thιιkɛ na ιnanι, kɛ sι-n mιιnι gιra'.
58002006	Mee ʋkha ka kɔɔ mιιrɛ dιkhãa pa Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ga thιmιι ayι: “Anye tibil do dι fι jιnaa dι tibil bιsaan gι dι fa hιιn?
58002007	Fι kɔɔ wuruure bɔɔ gbe dι 'lũ a jɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ. Fι kɔɔ haarɛ i dʋbιrɛ na cʋrɛ.
58002008	Fι cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ jʋʋraa dɩ jəəro nɛɛ.” Gɩdonɩ mɔ̃ Thãgbara cʋʋnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dιι jʋʋraa, thɩ̃ɛ na hale kpιιrakɛ sιι do ga jʋʋraa gaaga. Sιrakɛ sa yιɛ nɛnɛ̃ pι mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra jʋʋraana'.
58002009	Sι Jeju sι yι, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛɛkɛra Thãgba kɔɔ wurni bɔɔ gbe dι 'lũ a jɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ, dι mɛ̃ a na puno na khi tιbιla fɛʋʋ sora, gɩ do Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ dɔ nɔɔ, sɩ nɛnɛ̃ sɩ yɩɩrɛ mɔ̃ a 'lɛnɩ i dʋbɩrɛ na cʋrɛ, dɩɩ do khirikɛra a kɔɔ khini dɔ nɔɔ.
58002010	Mɔ̃ Thãgba na fʋnɩ sɩɩ do a cʋʋrɛ bikona jɔɔ dɩ wɩ 'lɛ i dʋbɩrɛ, gɛr gɩ dɩɩ tee kha dɩ ɔrkɛra tenɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, kɛ fɔnɩ dakha thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dɩɩ jɩɩl, kɔɔ gba bɔ gaarɛ a leena khal khaa ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ wa 'lɛrɔnɩ taarɛ.
58002011	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛnɩ tibil dɩ phu, na wɩrɛɛkɛ phonɩ, Thɩ bɩɛlla wɩ the fɛʋ, gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ yicuru na-n fʋ Jeju mɔ̃ a na we wɩnɩ õkona ga.
58002012	Dɩ gɩ har mɔna a sonɩ ayɩ: “Ma-n mɩɩrɛ ɩ̃ õkuunsɔ afɩda, ma-n khɩɩ fɛr kpa jɛdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn.”
58002013	Wo: “Mɛrɛ ma faarɛ ɩ̃ ha a na ha Thãgba.” Wo: “Mɛr ha ʋ na bɩsanaakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ha mɩnɩ.”
58002014	Gɛr gɩ gɩrɛ gɩdonɩ tɔmɩn na tomɩr bɩsana n hana, mɛ̃ Jeju kɔɔ hana gɩ dakha a puno a khi gɩ kʋkʋʋl ʋrɛ hιnanι fãgaakɛ dɔnι khidaa, ɔr dɔ Satã;
58002015	dι mɛ̃ Jejura na-n taa wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ khir n kʋnι maar dιι do dee paar gι pɛ wι awι yi hanana fɛʋ.
58002016	Gιdonι sobɔr gι, ga do thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ dɔ wιrɛ a na-n bulnə', sι gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “Abιrahamι məlsɔ dɔ wιrɛ a na-n bulni.”
58002017	Gɛr dɔ kιrʋ dιι tee kha dι kɔɔ debi a ho ɔɔ õkuunsɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, dι mɛ̃ a do gbõdaarιkɛ na-n jιɛnnι tibil bʋɔra, kɛ dɔnι sobɔdaar Thãgbaa thɔna, a na-n do sopugo hɛl thɔma tιbιlala.
58002018	Gιdonι mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ yιnι gaarɛ fifiləlela fɛʋʋkɛ a kɔɔ yɩnɩ, a hananɛ punone a na-n bulnə wιrɛ n yɛnι fifiləle.
58003001	Gɛr gι, omi phuusɔ, nɛrɛɛkɛ dakha Thãgba wenι, na-n hιnɛ Jejuukɛ a thɔnι dι do gbõdaar asι ha pɛdara,
58003002	kɛ dɔnι sobɔ cʋʋ tibil Thãgbaraakɛ kɔɔ pιɛraanι mɔ̃kɛ Mʋιjι dakha kɔɔ donι sobɔ cʋʋ tibil Thãgbaa cɔra fɛʋ.
58003003	Gιdonι gι teenaanɛ mɔ̃ a 'lɛnι i dʋbιrɛ a jɔ Mʋιjι mɔ̃kɛ cɔ mι n 'lɛnι ire dι jɔ cʋɔr thɛthɛ.
58003004	Cʋɔr wo cʋɔr sι mιmι n hale, dι ʋrɛ mɛnι thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ Thãgba gι.
58003005	Sι Mʋιjι wer mɔ̃ a donι thɔ̃ don, a dor sobɔ cʋʋ tibil Thãgbaa cɔra fɛʋ, gι do gιrɛ n nɛnanι gιrɛ teananι gι mιa.
58003006	Mɛ̃ Kirisiti ha dakha ɔɔ cɔ, sι Bikuun or do; dι ɔɔ cɔra sɛr gι, ado sι jιɛ fʋrɔ tu jιιrιkɛ sι hananι dιι ma, na nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ sι-n kãkarɔnι.
58003007	Gɛr gι, gι har mɔ̃kɛ Thu Phuu sonι ayι: “Nĩ, ado nι nιɛ ɔɔ wi,
58003008	na-n do anɩda n khɩɩr mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ hanɩ bɔɔraakɛ nɩ kɔɔ ɩɩrnanaanɩ cɩ̃cɩmanɛ, na bɔɔraalera nɩ kɔɔ fifiləəni bəənnə a hɩɩna'.
58003009	Liir anɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ kɔɔ fifilə mi a hɩɩn, wɩ kɔɔ jʋʋr mer a hɩɩn, sɩ wɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ mɔ̃ ɩ̃ thɔ̃ hanɩ a cʋʋna yɛna kpalanyɔ.
58003010	Gɛr gɩ dɩ nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋ mɩ wa bɔɔ tibil casɔraale, dɩ ɩ̃ so ayɩ: Kpɩɛrɛ lɛ̃ wɛr waa khorr; wa kɔɔ jɩ ɩ̃ hʋa'.
58003011	Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ ʋlfɛ mɔ̃ nĩkhii fʋ mɩnɩ ayɩ: Wa lõ ĩ hɩɩrra kpɩɩraka'.”
58003012	Omɩna, na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn dɩ tibil anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn na-n hana ha puukɛ dɔnɩ so bo haar, a ba kɛr a bir sa faa Thãgba yidaara'.
58003013	Sɩ na-n kpãkpaanɛ kha bɩɛlbɩɛl wire wire, mɔ̃ na punoni na so nayɩ: “Nĩkɛ”, gɩ do mɛ̃ tibil na ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn sopugo n fɩɩlʋʋ ɔɔda n khɩɩra'.
58003014	Gɩdonɩ sɩ debire a do wɩrɛ hɩnanɩ kha na Kirisiti gɩrɛ a hananɩ, ado sɩ jɩɛ fʋ kĩkĩ a dana khu paar tu jɩɩrɩkɛ sɩ kɔɔ hananɩ caca fʋ paar,
58003015	mɔ̃kɛra gɩ kherenɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Nĩ, ado nɩ nɩɛ ɔɔ wi, na-n do anɩda n khɩɩr mɔ̃kɛ gɩ kɔɔ hanɩ bɔɔraakɛ nɩ kɔɔ ɩɩrnanaanɩ cɩ̃cɩmana'.”
58003016	Gɩdonɩ ana dɔ wɩrɛɛkɛra kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ sa ɩɩrnanaa cɩ̃cɩmanɛ? Ga do wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛra Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ kpanɩ dɩ wɩ the Ejipiti dɩɩra gaa?
58003017	Dɩ anara nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋ Thãgba yɛna kpalanyɔ saagado wɩrɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ sopugo a thii le bəənnə ga?
58003018	Dɩ anara a kɔɔ ʋlfɛ ayɩ, wa lõ ɩnɩ hɩɩrra ga, ga do wɩrɛ kɔɔ nʋrɛnɩ nũu gaa?
58003019	Mɛ̃ sɩ yɩɛ dɩ wa kɔɔ puno a lõa' gɩdonɩ wɩ 'leere ha pɛrɛ.
58004001	Nɛnɛ̃ gɩrɛ, ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛna sɩnɩ sɩ lona ɩnɩ hɩɩrra, gɩ hale 'lo, gɛr gɩ dɔ maar na-n fʋ sɩ tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra na-n 'lee ga hɩɩrɩla'.
58004002	Gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ sɛr tutugo bʋɔɔ thɩmɩɩ mɔ̃kɛ wɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩnɩ, sɩ thɩmɩɩrɩlera wɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ ga kɔɔ cʋʋ wɩ thɩ̃a', gɩdonɩ ga kɔɔ caanna ha pɛrɛ wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛna'.
58004003	Sɩ ado sɛrkɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar gɩ, sɩ lʋʋn ɔɔ hɩɩrra, mɔ̃kɛra a sonɩ ayɩ: “Gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ ʋlfɛ mɔ̃ nĩkhii fʋ mɩnɩ ayɩ: Wa lõ ɩ̃ hɩɩrra kpɩɩraka'.” Sιι dorakɛ a fʋna bɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ tini thιι ɔɔ thɔ̃ kɔɔ mãa pιrɛ.
58004004	Gιdonι gι mιιrɛ pa bιɛl ɔɔ sɛbɛra wire makonyɔɔda ayι: “Wire makonyɔra Thãgba kɔɔ hιιr ɔɔ thɔnaakɛra fɛʋ a kɔɔ cʋʋnι.”
58004005	Dι a bire so ga thιmιιra ayι: “Wa lõ ɩ̃ hιιrra kpιιraka'.”
58004006	Hʋɛ phιnɛ dιphã casι ιkhasɔra dι wa puno na lõ ga hιιrraale, dι gιdonι wιrɛ kɔɔ dɔnι cacadaraakɛ kɔɔ nιɛnɛnι tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι, nũ nʋʋrɛ kɔɔ dor nɔɔ dι wa lõa',
58004007	Thãgba bire gιrɛ dιphã a pɛr wi kpιι wo, kɛ ɔɔ i n donι “Nĩkɛ”, dι gι ιnι na pʋɔr a cʋʋrɛ Davɩdɩ dɩ mɩɩ ga thɩmɩɩkɛ kɔɔ sɔnɩ ayɩ: “Nĩ, ado nɩ nɩɛ ɔɔ wi, na-n do anɩda n khɩɩra'.”
58004008	Gɩdonɩ ado Jojue kɔɔ ha wɛr hɩɩrɛ, gele pɩrɔnɩ Thãgba na bir na mɩɩ wi kpɩɩda bã.
58004009	Sɩ hɩɩrɛ hale wire makonyɔ wire Thãgba thɩɩnnɩ ɔɔ toora.
58004010	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ lonanɩ Thãgbaa hɩɩrra, a-n hɩɩrɛ dakha ɔɔ thɔna mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba hɩɩrnɩ ɔɔdara.
58004011	Gɛr gɩ sɩ yɩra a lona hɩɩrɛraale, dɩ tibil bɩɛl na-n lõ ga nũ nʋʋr caraale a 'lea'.
58004012	Gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa so hananɛ yire, gɩ-n cʋʋrɛ dakha thɩ̃ɛ, gɩ-n kher a jɔ bajɩna wo bajɩnaakɛ n khɛnɩ ƴɩɛ yenyɔ, gɩ-n gɔr phaphapha dɩɩ tɩnɛ haar na thue, dɩɩ tɩnɛ ƴɔɔ pa na khuu niin, gɩ-n pəlle tibili bɩ̃ na ɔɔ ha kpɩɛr.
58004013	Thɩ̃ bɩɛl na hale a ker dɩ aa yɩ gaaga, sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ toore gbelẽ gbelẽ a yɩr casɩ ɔɔ ƴɛra, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ sa mɩɩrɔnɩ asɩda.
58004014	Mɛ̃ gɩ gɩdonɩ sɩ hananɛ gbõdaar kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛlɩkɛ kɔɔ kpãsɛnɛnɩ thãgbara ƴũ, kɛ dɔnι Jeju Thãgbaa Bikuun, sι jιɛ jιιl kιbι ha pɛrɛraakɛ sι canι.
58004015	Gιdonι gbõdaarιkɛ sι hananι, ga do gbõdaar gιιkɛ na-n punoneni a na-n pər asι yɔɔra gaaga, sι ɔr, a kɔɔ yɩrɛ fifiləle asɩ kha thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra, sɩ aa cʋʋ sopugoə'.
58004016	Gɛr gɩ sa-n wɔrɔnɛ na tu jɩɩr Thãgbaa fãga too pa, ka bɔ jɩɩr hanɩ, mɛ̃ sa 'lɛ bɔ donanɛ, sa-n 'lɛna dakha bulle thɩ̃ ɓɔr bɔɔ ga-n the ɔɔ bɔ jɩra.
58005001	Gɩdonɩ gbõdaar wo gbõdaarɩkɛ wɩ-n phiirni tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, wɩ-n pɩɛraarɛ a na-n dɔ tɩbɩlala Thãgbaa thɔ̃, a na 'laana khaardaasɔ a na jenə bonɩɛ tɩbɩlaa sopugosɔra.
58005002	A-n dor ʋrɛ na-n hananɩ hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ yʋ 'leedarara, na wɩrɛraakɛ lɛnanɩ hʋɛra, gɩdonɩ a dor tibil dakha a yɔɔ.
58005003	Dɩ yɔɔrɛɛlera dɔ nɔɔ dɩɩ teena a je bonɩɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ sopugosɔra dakha mɔ̃kɛ a-n jini tɩbɩlaadara.
58005004	Tibil bɩɛl na hale na ti dɩbara nayɩ, ɩnɛr na cʋɛ thɔ̃ caale saagado Thãgba wɩɛ mɔ̃ a wenɩ Aarɔ̃ dɩ ha gaaga.
58005005	Mɛ̃ gɩ ha na Kirisiti. Ga do ɔr kɔɔ te ire dɩbara ɩnɩ-n dɔ gbõdaara', sɩ a 'lɛ gɛr ʋrɛraakɛ kɔɔ sʋɔraanɩ ayɩ: “Fɛr dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuun, mɛr Thãgba kɔna fɩ nĩ gɩrɛ.”
58005006	Mɔ̃kɛ a sonɩ dakha pa kpɩɩ wo ayɩ: “Fɛr dʋɔn bonɩ jidaar khorr mɔ̃kɛ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩɩ kpam hanɩ.”
58005007	Ɔɔ yi hana bɔɔ kɛ thɩɩra, khɩɩ khena na yilẽbe a kɔɔ bɩɛlna Thãgba da-n ƴɛɛnaa, ɔrkɛ hananɩ punone na taanaa khirrə, dɩ ɔɔ dɩbara jo dor nɔɔ dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ tu ɔɔ bɩɛl.
58005008	A donɩnakɛ Bikuun sɩ a kɔɔ dɩɩrɛ nũ nɩɩr dɩɩ the gɩrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ gaarɔnɩ bʋɔ.
58005009	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ a danɩ waa thu pɩ, a debire do khorr taa 'lɛ paar wɩrɛraakɛ n nɩɛnɛɛnɩ nũu;
58005010	dɩ Thãgba kɔɔ pɩɛrɛ a dɔ gbõdaar mɔ̃kɛ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩɩ kpam hanɩ.
58005011	Ga thɩmɩɩra sɩ hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ a na mɩɩ, sɩ thɩ̃ɛ gɩɩkɛ khiinoni mɩɛrɛra gɩdonɩ anɩ nũ ka hulone.
58005012	Gɩdonɩ nɛrɛɛkɛ kɛkɛkɛ kanɩ teena nɩ deba dɔ tɩbɩlaa dɩɩrdara, nɛr ha wɩrɛ 'lo n ƴaalɛnɩ wɩ birə na dɩrɛ nɩ Thãgbaa so tɔ̃tʋ̃ɔ pa, dɩɩ do ɩlɛ̃ nɩ-n ƴaal 'lo na-n ƴaal dɩko khena ga.
58005013	Dɩ tibilikɛ n bɔnɩ da-n jɩɩl ɩlɛna, aa-n jɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ dasarʋ kpɩa', gɩdonɩ bɩsã buu a do.
58005014	Sɩ dɩko khena wɩrɛ bɩnanɩ hɩna, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ mɩlananɩ bɩ̃ kuure, dɩ wɩ puno dɩ wa-n jɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ na gɩrɛ puuroni.
58006001	Gɛr gɩ dɔ sɩ sɩrɔ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ Kirisitii thɩmɩɩ tɔ̃tʋ̃ɔ pa, sɩ sɩ bãba sa-n ƴaal dɩɩrɛɛkɛ na cʋɛ sɩnɩ dɩ sa bɩ̃; sa-n bir 'lo a na jɩɩl gɩrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ tɔ̃tʋ̃ɔ paar, kɛ dɔnɩ thɔ̃ khi faarɛ, na ha pɛrɛ Thãgbara ga,
58006002	na dɩɩrɛ yɔ kpɛɛrɛsɔra na nyɛ̃ dɛɛna', na khee ɩɩr na khorr kɩɩla'.
58006003	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ sa cʋʋnɩ a Thãgba tu.
58006004	Gɩdonɩ ado wɩrɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ Thãgbaa dahɩrɛ gɩ, kɛ 'lɛnɩ khaardaakɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ a hɩɩn, kɛ 'lɛnɩ dakha awɩda Thu Phuurə,
58006005	a 'lɛna dakha Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩkɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ a hɩɩn, na fãgaakɛ dɔnɩ bɔɔkɛ n ɩnanɩɩda;
58006006	a tibil ca wele kɛr bir, wa puno na bir na debi haar bã, gɩdonɩ we wer wɩ bire gba Thãgbaa Bikuun dɩ wa-n kpa kʋkʋ thɩrʋra, dɩɩ do yicuru wɩ-n pɩɛraa tɩbɩlaa ƴɛra.
58006007	Thɩɩkɛ thãgba nyʋɔn n sɛnɩ wire wire dɩ phu thɩ̃ khonanɛ wɩrɛraakɛ kʋlɛɛnɩ, Thãgba bɔnanɛ a 'lɛ.
58006008	Sɩ ado a phu uu na sɩkajɩɩl, bɔ taa thɩɩ gι bã, sɔ̃ togʋʋ a too dɩ pɩpɩɩ paar dɔɔ a na caanna.
58006009	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, sɩ-n mɩɩnɩnakɛ thakɛ sɩ sɩ hana narɛ tu jɩɩr dɩ nɩ har hʋ bʋɔraakɛ dɔnɩ taa hʋɛ.
58006010	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba na gõgolõ a na diinə anɩ thɔ̃ na naʋʋkɛ nɩ-n nɩnanɩ ɔɔ irə, mɔ̃kɛ nɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnι thɩ̃ɛ ɔɔ tιι phusɔra a ba harakɛ cʋʋrɔ gιra'.
58006011	Sι-n ƴaalɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl n hanana ga gbɛ̃gbɛrɛ̃ ca gι dana khu paar; dι mɛ̃ gιrɛ nι-n pɛnι nũu na dã na ha otirə.
58006012	Sa-n ƴaal dokhʋʋr n fɔ na', sι na-n phɛla wιrɛ 'lɛnι gιrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛna wιnι ιna ha wɛr, gι the awι ha pɛra na awι ha fʋra.
58006013	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanι Abιraham, gι hʋrɛ nʋɔ gι dι so, dι ire na hanιle a kɔ̃tɩ̃ jɔ ɔɔda dι na wa', ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ i a we a sona nʋɔɔle,
58006014	ayι: “Sobɔr gι, ma bɔna fɛr dι a kɔ̃tɩ̃, dι ma cʋʋrɛ afι məl dι wa ler na jɔr.”
58006015	Thale Abιraham n kɔɔ pιɛr na ha fʋrɛ a 'lɛ gιrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnaanι ιna haarɛ.
58006016	Tιbιla ireekɛ kãasιnɛnι awιdara wι-n soro nʋɔ, dι thɩ̃ banaa fɛʋʋkɛ hanι awι thɩ̃thιιn ga pιrɛ nɔ sorraale.
58006017	Dι gɛr gι mɔ̃ Thãgba n ƴaalnι a jιι nιna ɔɔ ʋlfɛ 'lɛdara dι gιrɛ a pɛrnι haar ιna cʋʋrɛ na do daphιlanaa ga, gɛr gι dι ɓaan nɔ sor.
58006018	Dι mɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛ yenyɔɔkɛ na dɔnι daphιlanaa ga, kɛ Thãgba na punoni na kuro sõsora', na cʋʋ sι dι sa hana 'lar dι a jɔr na ka, sɛrkɛ asι phι pa donι nũ pɛ hananɛ gιrɛraakɛ thιnɛ sarnι ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ.
58006019	Ga nũ pɛ caakɛ sι hananι gι hʋrɛ gborõ fʋ therιkɛ n fɔnι gborõo dιɩ ma, gɩ-n kpãsɛrɛ kɩ̃kɩɩnna dɩɩ lõ a dã bɩnɔ,
58006020	ka Jejn do sarnɩ ƴɛ kʋl a lõ mɔ̃ a donɩ gbõdaar khorr mɔ̃kɛ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩɩ kpam hanɩ.
58007001	Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩ ʋrɛra Salɛm fãgadaar gɩ, a dona Thãgba Kəkəədaarɩ bonɩ jidaar, ɔr kɔɔ caanɛ Abɩraham ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ punoni fãgadara sɩ da-n ɩ̃, dɩ a kɔɔ bɔnanɛ Abɩraham;
58007002	dɩ Abɩraham haarɛ bɩɛl yʋɔrra ɔɔ thɩ̃sɔra fɛʋ. “Fɩl sar fãgadaar” a do mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ i kɩr hanɩ, wo Salɛm fãgadaar a do dakha, a thɩɛna gaa “ha ie fãgadaar” gɩ.
58007003	Aa hana thɩra', aa hana nɩra', aa hana məllə'; ɔɔ yi na hana fʋ paara', ga hana pɩ paara'; Thãgbaa Bikuun a ho, a too khorr a do bonι jidaar.
58007004	Hιnɛ mɔ̃kɛ kuunile kɔ̃tιnι, ʋrɛɛkɛra asι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abιraham kɔɔ tini bιɛl yʋɔr ɔɔ thιna a ha, kɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ a thenanɩ kʋʋrra.
58007005	Levɩɩ bɩsã ɩkhaakɛ n dɔnɩ bonɩ ji thɔma, jɔfʋ ha wɛr hʋɛ dɩ wa tee bɩɛl yʋɔr tɩbɩlala, a thɩɛna gaa awɩ omisɔra wɛ, kɛrakɛ dɔnɩ Abɩrahamɩ məlsɔ.
58007006	Sɩ ɔrkɛra na thɛnɩ awɩ thɩ kɔna ga, a teere Abɩraham bɩɛl yʋɔrra, dɩ a kɔɔ bɔnanɛ ʋrɛ ʋlfɛrɛ telenɩ.
58007007	Dɩ bananɛ na hala', ʋrɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ n bɔna ʋrɛ 'lunoni.
58007008	Mɔ̃ gɩ-n hanɩ gbõdaraa pa, tɩbɩlaakɛ dɔnɩ wɩ-n khire, wɛr n tea bɩɛl yʋɔrra, sɩ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩ wer, kɛ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ yɩnɩ aa do dakhinənə', ɔr tea kɩɛr bɩɛl yʋɔrra.
58007009	Levɩɩkɛ n 'lɛnɩ bɩɛl yʋɔrra, sɩ punone so dɩ Abɩraham bɩɛl yʋɔrraakɛ a 'laanɩ ɔr 'laanɛ,
58007010	dɩ gɩdonɩ ɔɔ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abɩraham na kɔɔ kʋ̃ɔ sɩ dɩ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩ caanʋa'.
58007011	Levɩtɩɩ bonɩ ji thɔna jɔfʋʋkɛ tɩbɩla 'lɛnɩ kɔɔ ɩɩr, dɩ ado gɩ dor thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ a dã thu, anyera bonɩ jidaar kpɩɩ bir hale mɔ̃kɛ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩɩ kpam hanɩ, sɩ ga do wo mɔ̃kɛ Aarɔ̃ɔ kpam hanɩ ga?
58007012	Dɩ gɩdonɩ bonɩ ji thɔma debire, dɔ jɔfʋ n debi dakha.
58007013	Sɩ ʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ mɩɩrɔnɩ ca kpɩɩ gɩ, kɛrakɛ wa bɩɛl na-n kɔɔ donɩ thɔma bonɩ ji paara'.
58007014	Gɩ yɩrrɛ casɩ dɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Judaa cara a the, kɛ dɔnɩ caarɩkɛ Mʋɩjɩ na kɔɔ mɩɩnɩnakɛ dɩkha dɩɩ ɩɩna bonɩ jidaraada ga.
58007015	Gɩ jɩɛ yɩr casɩ dɩphã, gɩdonɩ bonɩ jidaar kpɩɩ ɩɩrɛ kɛ hɔnɩ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩ.
58007016	Ɔɔ bonɩ jidaar do, ga do mɔ̃ tibil jɔfʋ n pɛrnɩ gɩ hana mɛ̃ gɩ ha ga, sɩ yireekɛ na dɔnɩ dapɩnana', ga fãga a dona.
58007017	Gɩdonɩ gɩ mɩɩrɛ ɔɔda Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Fɛr dʋɔn bonɩ jidaar khorr mɔ̃kɛ Mɛlkɩsɛdɛkɩɩ kpam hanɩ.”
58007018	Mɛ̃ gɩ dɩ mama jɔfʋ hɛllɔ, gɩdonɩ ga hana fãga ga, ga-n taa bʋɔ dakha ga,
58007019	jɔfʋ na-n cʋʋnɩ tibil dɩ bɔr dɩ dã thuə', sɩ nũ pɛrɛɛkɛ baannɩ ɩnɛ dɩphã, gɛr dʋɔn gɩrɛ sɩ-n wɔrɔnanɩ Thãgba.
58007020	Dɩ gɩdonɩnakɛ thɩ̃ɛ thale na kɔɔ dã sɩ ga do nɔ so ʋlfɛrɛ haanɔaa ga, sɩ Levɩtɩsɔ wer dor bonɩ jidara sɩ nɔ so ʋlfɛrɛ na hala'.
58007021	Sɩ Jeju wer dor bonɩ jidaar na nɔ so ʋlfɛrɛ dɩ gɩ ther Thãgbaraakɛ sʋɔraanɩ ayɩ: “Mɛr Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ʋlfɛrɛ na nɔ sor, sɩ ma debi kpɩɛra' ayɩ: Fɛr dʋɔn bonɩ jidaar khorr.”
58007022	Nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ baannɩ a jɔ fĩi, Jeju doro ga barãda.
58007023	Dɩrakɛ wo bonɩ jidaraale wɩ-n jɔrɛ gɩdonɩ khir n dor nɔɔ dɩ wa-n pʋɔra'.
58007024	Sɩ gɩdonɩ o wer khorrdaar a do, a hɩnɛ bonɩ ji thɔmaakɛ na seerenɩ na ka tɩɩ kpɩɩra ga.
58007025	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ da puno na taa waa vʋ̃ʋ wιrɛ na kanι ɔɔ pa sι na yι hʋɛ a na wɔrɔ̃ Thãgba, gιdonι yidaar a do khorr dι ƴɛɛna Thãgba da-n pɛ war.
58007026	Dι gι teere kha sι hananι gbõdaar caa thale dι phu, a do dι pa 'leedaar, aa hana jiinə', a leere kpιι na sopugodara; thãgbara ƴũukɛ gbaanɛnι sι ɔɔda kãasι garɛ.
58007027	Aa hana ƴaalɛ wɩ̃ gbõdaraa kha a na-n ji bonιɛ wire koo ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ sopugosɔra ɓo sι a ji a na-n pɛ tιbιlala ga, gιdonι babιɛl a kɔɔ jinə dιbara bonιɛ mɔ̃ a kɔɔ 'laanι ɔɔbara.
58007028	Gιdonι jɔfʋ n pɛrɛ tιbιlaakɛ dɔnι yɔyɔa dι wι do gbõdara, sι Thãgbaa ʋlfɛ nɔ sookɛ pιrɔnι a kpa jɔfʋra kɔɔ pιɛr Bikuun waa khorr, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ dananι thu.
58008001	Gιrɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι gιrɛraakɛ sι-n sonι gɛr dʋɔn, sι hananɛ le Thãgbaa dʋɔ gbõdaar caalera tɔɔnι Thãgba dawabʋʋ fãgadaar too para nyɔ̃bɔɔra,
58008002	da-n do thɔma Thãgba fʋɔr paarιkɛ dɔnι kẽkẽ wa bɔɔkɛ Kɔ̃tιnι thɛthɛ kɔɔ dʋnι, ga do tibil doa'.
58008003	Gbõdaar wo gbõdaarιkɛ wι-n pɛrnι, wι-n pιɛrɛ a na-n 'laanɛ khaardaa Thãgbara a na jenə bonιɛ, dι gɛr gι gι teenanɛ asι gbõdaar n hanana dakha thɩ̃ɛ a 'laanɛ.
58008004	Ado thιιra a kɔɔ ha, a na kɔɔ do bonι jidaara', gιdonι wɛ hale n 'laanɛnι khaardaa mɔ̃ jɔfʋ sonι.
58008005	Dι bonι jidaraale gιrɛ wι-n cʋʋnι gι hʋrɛ gιrɛ hanι Thãgbaa dʋɔ dι ga jəər gi; mɛ̃ gι kɔɔ ha na Mʋιjι ɔbɔɔkɛ a-n dʋnι kẽkẽ waa, Thãgba sʋʋraarɛ ayι: “Jιɛ hιιn, sa cʋɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ gι ho gιrɛ fι kɔɔ yιnι gɔ̃gʋɔna.”
58008006	Sι nɛnɛ̃ Kirisiti 'lɛr thɔmaakɛ kɔ̃tιnanι a jɔ awιda fɛʋ, mɔ̃kɛ a donι ƴɛƴɛɛ dιι do nɔɔ dι nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ baannι hale, kɛ jιlɛnι ʋlfɛ thɩmɩɩrraakɛ baannɩ dakha.
58008007	Gɩdonɩ ado caca nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛ 'leere dɩ paar, anyera wa ƴaal balanyɔdaa 'lo?
58008008	Sɩ dɩɩkɛ Thãgba yɩ warnɩ a soro thakɛ ayɩ: “Mɛr Kɔ̃tɩn sɔ ayɩwɔɔ: Wire hale na dã, dɩ ma ʋlfɛ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ phaa na Ɩjɩrayɛl ca na Judaa ca dakha;
58008009	ga ho nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ ƴιrɛ mɩ kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ awɩ mama thɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, bɔɔraalera mɩ kɔɔ fʋ wɩnɩ na nyɛ̃ɛ a ti Ejipiti dɩɩra ga. Dɩ gɩdonɩ wɛr thɛthɛ na kɔɔ bãba ɩ̃ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛra a jιι fʋ ga, mɛrɛ dakha ma kɔɔ pər wara', mɛr Kɔ̃tιn sɔ.
58008010	Kɔ̃tιn sɔ ayɩwɔɔ: A ga wiile dã, nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ ma ʋlfɛnanɩ Ɩjɩrayɛl ca, thakɛ ga ha: Ma pɛrɛ ɩ̃ jɔfʋsɔ awɩ kpɩɛrra, ma khere ger awɩ hara; ma dor awɩ Thãgba, wɩ do ɩ̃ too.
58008011	Tibil na hana a dɩɩr ʋrɛ wɩ khunəni kha, dɩ õkuun gɩ a na-n dɩɩr õkuun a so ayɩ: Jɛ Kɔ̃tɩna'. Gɩdonɩ fɛʋ na jɩ mɛr, gɩ fʋna tɩɩ pɔɩ gɩ gbana tɩɩ kɔ̃tɩna.
58008012	Gɩdonɩ ma jɩ wɛr bʋɔra awɩ thɩ̃ gõgolona, dɩrakɛ ma jɩna awɩ sopugosɔ kpɩɩ bã.”
58008013	Mɔ̃ a-n wenɩ ʋlfɛrɛɛle daphaa, a cʋʋrɛ cacadaa dɩɩ do datɩ̃ɩ. Dɩ gɩrɛ tɩnanɩ a kpɔrɔ n jaal gɩrɛ bũburõ paar.
58009001	Dɩ caca nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛra dakha kɔɔ hananɛ jɔfʋsɔ mɔ̃kɛ tɩbɩla na fʋɔrnɩ Thãgba, a hanana dakha Thãgba fʋɔr paar kɛ thɩɩra.
58009002	Gɩdonɩ kẽkẽ waa kɔɔ dʋrɛ, dɩ ka wɩ-n kɔɔ lonɩ dã caca le wɩ-n we pa phuu; liir dɔ carã dɛ̃ɛ paar kɔɔ ha, na tabal, na buruukɛ wɩ-n hanɩ Thãgba.
58009003	Sɩ balanyɔ kẽkẽ billo liir dɔ paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ sãsɩ pa phuu,
58009004	dɛ bʋlaa hale kɛ dɔnɩ latɩkolo 'wii paar, na nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ khɛɛsʋʋkɛ wɩ kolnɩ koo na dɛ kãkɛ dɛ bʋlaakɛ wɩ pɛrnɩ maan hanɩ, na kãkɛ Aarɔ̃ɔ gbolɩkɛ kɔɔ phɛnɩ phɩ̃ɩ hanɩ, na bokanaakɛ wɩ khereronɩ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ thɩmɩɩr.
58009005	Nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ khɛɛsʋʋra ƴũule thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ hale kɛ n nɛnanɩ Thãgbaa i dʋbɩ, dɩ awɩ jəər n kɔɔ kɛa so hɛl paar; sɩ ga do ga thɩmɩɩsɔ sɩ-n ƴaal sɩ mɩɩ nɩ nɛnɛ̃ kɩrʋ n yɩra'.
58009006	Dɩ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔlera hanɩ thale, bonɩ jidara n lʋʋn bɔɔ fɛʋ caca paar waaraale dɩ wa-n do awɩ thɔ̃.
58009007	Sɩ balanyɔ paar gbõdaar dɩbara n lona babɩɛl yɛ bɩɛl. Tɔmɩnɩkɛ a jinəni bonɩɛ a pɛ ɔɔbara na tɩbɩlaa sopugosɔra a-n lona.
58009008	Gɛr dɔ gɩrɛ Thu Phuu nɩnanɩ dɩ sãsɩ pa phu hʋɛ na khɛr pɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ caca kẽkẽ waa hanɩle 'loa'.
58009009	Sokpaa gɩ dɩ ga-n nɩ sar mɔ̃kɛ thɩ̃ɛ hanɩ nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ, dɩ khaardaasɔ na bonɩɛɛkɛ wɩ-n jini, ga puno na cʋʋ tibilikɛ n fʋɔrɛnɩ Thãgba thale, gɩ do ɔɔ kpɩɛrnɔ bɔrɛ waa a dã thuə'.
58009010	Gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ khonanɛ gɩ, na dayɔnanɛ, na phʋɔl caarsɔ dɩɩdɩɩ dɩbara, kɛ tɩbɩla pɛrnɩ dɩɩ do jɔfʋ phaphapha gɩ dana bɔɔkɛ Thãgba na gbɛbɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ dɩ ga jɩɩ bɔr.
58009011	Sɩ Kirisiti ɩnɛ a do gbõdaar thɩ̃ bʋɔraakɛ hanɩkɛ gɩrɛ; a kɔɔ kpãsɛrɛ waaraakɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ ka, kɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ dakha ka, kɛ na dɔnɩ tibili nyɛ̃ thɔ̃a', kɩrʋ dʋɔn, ga do thɩɩkɛɛda ga.
58009012	A kɔɔ lʋʋn babιɛl khorr sãsɩ pa phuurə sɩ ga do bʋ tɔmɩn na na ɓol tɔmɩn a kɔɔ lona ga, sɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ tɔmɩ̃ gɩ, dɩɩ do babɩɛl a kɔɔ birse si waa khorr.
58009013	Gɩdonɩ ado bʋ tɔmɩn, na nake tɔmɩn, na naphɩɩ thookɛ wɩ-n gbanɩ a jɛbɩ wɩrɛraakɛ biseneni dɩɩ do gɩ phʋɔl wɛr dɩ wɩ phu gɩdonɩ wɩ lɩrɛ,
58009014	mɔ̃ ga ka na ha na gɩrɛ Kirisitii tɔmɩ̃ n cʋʋnι, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ kɔɔ 'laanɛnι ɔɔbara Thãgbara a do bonι jirikɛ na hananι sι paara', dιι do Thu Phuukɛ dɔnι khorrdaarι pa gι the. Kirisitii tɔmɩ̃ιlera na phʋɔlɛ asι ha a na ti mɔlɔ thɔmaakɛ sι kɔɔ cʋʋnι sι sι puno dιphã sa-n fʋɔr Thãgba yidaar.
58009015	Gɛr gι dι Kirisiti do ƴɛƴɛɛ dιι do nɔɔ dι nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛ phaa hale, dι mɛ̃ wιrɛ Thãgba wenι na puno na 'lɛ bɔnanɛɛkɛ dɔnι khorrdaa, kɛ Thãgba yιnι ιna 'laarɛ. Gι punone ha mɛ̃ gιdonι bιɛl kɔɔ khire dι khirile na birsene tιbιla dι wa the puureraakɛ wι kɔɔ cʋʋnι caca nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛ bɔɔ.
58009016	Gιdonι a thɩ̃ gba sɛbɛ hale, dɔ tue n jι dι ʋrɛ kheranι sɛbɛɛlera khire.
58009017	Gιdonι thɩ̃ gba sɛbɛɛle na-n taa bʋɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ kheranι hananι yirə', sι gι-n taarɛ bʋɔ bɔɔkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ kheranι khini pι dιphã.
58009018	Gɛr dɔ kιrʋ dι caca nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛrɛ na kɔɔ puno na jιɩ do ʋlfɛrɛ sɩɩ do tɔmɩn na kɔɔ halaa ga.
58009019	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Mʋɩjɩ kɔɔ sonɩ jɔfʋ sɛbɛra jɔfʋ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ ƴɛra pɩ, a gbaar bana sũu sɩɛ, na ɩjopɩ faa, a ɓɛna na ɓol tɔmɩn na bʋ tɔmɩn, na nyʋɔn a jɛbɩ sɛbɛraale na tɩbɩlala fɛʋ sa so ayɩ:
58009020	“Tɔmɩnɩkɛ dʋɔn nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ jɩɩn nɛrɛra na Thãgba.”
58009021	Ɔmɛna a jɛbɩ dakha tɔmɩn kẽkẽ waara, na Thãgba fʋɔr thɔ̃ do thɩ̃ɛsɔra fɛʋʋkɛ hanιle.
58009022	Ado jɔfʋra gι, gι sɩrɛ fɩɩʋrakɛ sɩɩ do thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ tɔmɩn n phʋɔlɛ gɩ, dɩ ado tɔmɩn na deera', sopugo faarɛ na hala'.
58009023	Thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛra fɛʋ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ n nɛnanɩ mɔ̃ ƴũ thɩ̃ɛsɔ hanι, gι teenanɛ phʋɔlɛ thakɛ, dɩ gɩrɛɛ thɛthɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ ƴũdaa bonɩ jirikɛ baannι gɩ-n ƴaal.
58009024	Gɩdonɩ Kirisiti na kɔɔ lõ pa phuurəəkɛ tibil nyɛ̃ɛ cʋʋna', kɛ n kporonanɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ bire, sɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔɔ thɛthɛ a lõ, dɩ mɛ̃ a na-n jɩɩl gɩrɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra asɩ jɩɩl.
58009025	Dɩ dakha wo aa-n kɔɔ lõ le da-n jinə ɔɔ dɩbara bonɩɛ bɔɔ fɛʋ, mɔ̃kɛ gbõdaar n lonɩ pa phuurə yɩɛr koo na thɩ̃ kpɩɩ tɔmã'.
58009026	Agado mɛ̃ ga, ga dor bɔɔ fɛʋra a na-n kɔɔ gaar bʋɔ gɩ fʋna thɩɩ ti bɔɔ; sɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ dɩphã pɩpɩɩ bɔɔraakɛ babɩɛl a kɔɔ ɩ̃ sopugo hɛl ɩɩn, gɩ the gɩrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ gbanɩ ɔɔbara a jinə bonɩɛ.
58009027	Tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛlɩda dʋɔn babɩɛl wa khi, agɩpɩ Thãgba n kɩɩlna wɩ.
58009028	Mɛ̃ dakha Kirisiti kɔɔ jinə dɩbara bonɩɛ babɩɛl a heen tibil jɔjʋɔɔ sopugo, sɩ balanyɔdaa a na bire na ɩ̃, ga do sopugodaara gɩ bã, sɩ wɩrɛ n pɩɛrɛɛnɩɩ taa pa gɩ mɛ̃.
58010001	Jɔfʋ na do thɩ̃ biree thɛtha', sɩ thɩ̃ ɓʋ̃ɔɔkɛ na ɩnanɩɩ jəər gɩ, dɩ a na puno kpɩɩrakɛ na bonɩ ji ca bɩɛlɩlera n jenɩsɔ wire wire yɩɛr koo, a na cʋʋ wɩrɛ n pɔnɩ Thãgbara dɩ wa bɔr na dã thuə'.
58010002	Gɩdonɩ ado wɩrɛ n fʋɔrɛnɩ Thãgba thale awɩ sopugosɔ kɔɔ hɛl warɛ sobɔr, ga dor sopugoo so heen fɩɩʋrakɛ na bo na too awɩ hara bã, dɩ wa sɩrɔrɛrakɛ dakha bonɩ jir.
58010003	Sɩ ga bonɩ jiile n ka cʋʋrɛ tɩbɩla yɩɛr koo dɩ wa-n jɩna awɩ sopugosɔ.
58010004	Gɩdonɩ nake tɔmɩn na bʋ tɔmɩn na puno na hɛl sopugosɔ kpɩɩraka'.
58010005	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ mɔ̃ Kirisiti n lonɩ kɛ thɩɩra a sor Thãgbara ayɩ: “Ga do bonɩ jir fɩ-n ƴaal dɩ khaardaa ga, sɩ tomɩr fɩ mɩ mɩ.
58010006	Nʋ̃ thii bonɩ jir, na sopugo hɛl bonɩ jir na-n da fara';
58010007	dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ so: Hɩnɛ mɛr ha ʋ, ɩ̃ cʋʋ afɩ tuur ya Thãgba, gɩ ha mɔ̃kɛ ɩ̃dara kherenɩ lo sɛbɛra.”
58010008	Gɩrɛ a sonɩ caca dʋɔn: “Ga do bonɩ jir fɩ-n ƴaal, dɩ khaardaa gɩ, dɩ nʋ̃ thii bonɩ jir gɩ, dɩ sopugo hɛl bonɩ jir ga, ga-n da fara'.” Sɩɩ do mɔ̃ jɔfʋ pɛrnɩ ga bonɩɩle n ji.
58010009	Agɩpɩ a sor wo: “Hɩnɛ mɛr ha ʋ ɩ̃ cʋʋ afι tuur.” Mɛ̃ a hɛllɔ caca bonι jir sι Kirisitii bonι ji lõ ga kara.
58010010	Gιdonι Jeju Kirisiti cʋʋrɛ gιrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ƴaalnι a cʋɛ a 'laa ɔɔ tomι babιɛl khorr, sι phu sι lee kpιɩ.
58010011	Bonɩ jidara fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl ƴũ jιιlɔ wι-n jιιl dι wa-n do awι thɔ̃ dι wa-n ji bonι ji ca bιɛlsɔra wire wire, kɛ na-n punoneni na ti sopugo kpιιraka'.
58010012	Sι o wer bonι ji bιɛl a kɔɔ ji sopugora sa too gιrɛ khorr Thãgbaa nyɔ̃bɔra,
58010013	da-n pιɛr dιphã phaphapha Thãgba n cʋʋ ɔɔ lãlaardara wɩ dʋʋraa ɔɔ nɛ jəəda.
58010014	Gιdonι bonι ji bιɛl a cʋʋna wιrɛ phonι a lee kpιι dι wι bɔr ka khorr a dã thu.
58010015	Dι Thu Phuu cʋʋ sɛr dakha dɩ sɩ jɩ tue. Cacara a sor ayɩ:
58010016	“Kɔ̃tɩn sɔ ayɩwɔɔ: A ga wiile dã, nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ ma ʋlfɛna wɩnɩ thakɛ ga ha: Ma pɛrɛ ɩ̃ jɔfʋsɔ awɩ hara, ma khere ger awɩ kpɩɛrra.”
58010017	Dɩ a sor wo: “Ma jɩna awɩ sopugosɔ dɩ awɩ thɩ̃ gõgolõ gɩ kpɩɩ bã.”
58010018	Dɩ ka sopugo faarɛ n hanɩ bonɩɛ na-n ji sopugora bã.
58010019	Mɛ̃ gɩ omɩna, sι jιrɛ tue dι hʋɛ phιnɛ dιphã waa dι sa-n lona sãsι pa phuurə, dιι do Jeju Kirisitii tɔmɩ̃ dɔ nɔɔ.
58010020	Hʋɛɛlera a kɔɔ phɛl sarnι hʋ phaa gι, a dona yi hʋɛ, a kpãsɛ kɩ̃kιιnna, a thιɛna gaa ɔɔ tomι gι.
58010021	Dι wo sι hananɛ gbõdaarιkɛ Thãgba pɛrnι dι do yʋʋ ɔɔ cɔ.
58010022	Mɛ̃ gɩ sɩ jɩɛ tɔ na wɔrɔ̃ Thãgba na ha bʋɔ, na ha pɛrɛɛkɛ dananɩ thu, na haarɩkɛ Thãgba phʋɔlnɩ a ti kpɩɛrnɔ puu a faa, a na wɔrɔnaa dakha na tomɩrɩkɛ cɔcɔɔnɛnɩ na yɔ hɩrɛ.
58010023	Sɩ fɔ asɩ nũ pɛɛkɛra sɩ yɩnɩ sɩ hananɛ kĩkĩ, gɩdonɩ sɩ jɩɛ jɩ tue dɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba ʋlfɛnɩ ɩna cʋʋrɛ, gɛrra a na cʋʋ.
58010024	Sa-n jɩɛ dʋ kha bʋrɛ gɩ tɔ naʋ ga-n pɛr na dakha thɔ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛ.
58010025	Sa-n bo pa bɩɛl gbɛbɩra', mɔ̃kɛ ɩkhasɔ n cʋʋna', sɩ sa-n mɩa kha yɩr thɩmɩa, mɔ̃ nɩ taanɩ yɩ Wireele dɩ ga-n wɔrɔ̃.
58010026	Gɩdonɩ a sɩ jɩ gbobi sɩ na cʋʋ sopugo ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ 'lini 'lɛr sobɔ jɩɩr pɩ, bonɩɛ na-n hale sopugora bã.
58010027	Sɩ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ ma kʋ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ sɛnɩ dʋɔn kɩɩlʋ na Thãgbaa ha kpor nĩkhiikɛ na thiəni ɔɔ lãlaardara dɔ khaa.
58010028	Tibil wo tibilikɛ n kɔɔ kʋɛanɩ Mʋɩjɩɩ jɔfʋ, ado tɩbɩla yenyɔ yẽthersɔ so ɩnɩ torre yire, wɩ-n kɔɔ kʋʋrɛ sι wa-n jιι bʋɔra ga.
58010029	Nι kpιɛrɛ hιnɛ mɔ̃ ga puuro na pɔna ʋrɛraakɛ na-n gbaannι Thãgbaa Bikuun dι dʋʋraa thɩ̃a', kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ n hιnɛnι nɔ bιɛl ʋlfɛ tɔmιnιkɛ phʋɔlɛɛnι dιι dʋʋraa mɔlɔ thɩ̃ɛ, da-n kpɛna dakha Thu Phuukɛ dɔnι bɔ jιdaa.
58010030	Gιdonι sι jιrɛ ʋrɛ kɔɔ sɔnι ayι: “Hel tiire dɔ ιnda, dι mɛr dɔ ʋrɛ na lιmanι tibil gιrɛ a cʋʋnι”, wo, “Kɔ̃tιn na kιιlnanɛ ɔɔ too.”
58010031	Thɩ̃ɛ gι dι ga-n kʋ maar ka ado fɩ təə ji Thãgba yidaarι nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
58010032	Na-n jɛna caca wiresɔ, ɔbɔɔkɛ nι kɔɔ 'lɛnι Thãgbaa dahιrɛ pι, nι kɔɔ jιιlɛ kιbι kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ kɔ̃tιιna bʋɔraakɛ nι-n gaarnι.
58010033	Kho bιɛl nι dor yι ga thɩ̃ɛ nιιrɛraakɛ wι-n nιιr nιnι na nιwɛraakɛ nι-n yιnι, kho bιɛl wo nι ture a lõ bɔ gaar bιɛlla na wιrɛɛkɛ n gaarɛnι thale.
58010034	Dι bʋɔ n kɔɔ fʋ nɛr wιrɛraakɛ dɔnι khaιdara, dι nι ture na daʋ tιbιla n taa nar thɩ̃ɛ, sι dι na-n jιna dι nι hananɛ thɩ̃ ƴιrɛ baannι a do thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n pʋɔrɛnι khorr.
58010035	Gɛr gι na-n dʋna anι tu jιra a fagaa koe, gι hananɛ khorιkɛ kɔ̃tιnanι tə̃ə.
58010036	Nι teenanɛ nι hanana yιrrɛ ado nι-n ƴaalɛ na-n cʋɛ gιrɛ Thãgba tuni, a 'lɛna gιrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnι a ha nι.
58010037	Gιdonι gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Kɩɛr na bɔɔ gbe fɩɩʋ, ʋrɛɛkɛra hanɩ ɩɩn da-n ɩ̃ a na daan a na pʋɔra';
58010038	sɩ ʋrɛ mɩ hɛllɔnɩ sor dɩɩ do ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ, ɔr na hana yire, sɩ ado a kɛr bir ɔɔda na da mar haara kpɩɩraka'.”
58010039	Sɩ se wer sa do wɛkɛ n kɛranɩ dɩ wɩ bir khiro a na buurə', sɩ sɛr dɔ wɛkɛ hananɩ ha pɛrɛ gɩ taa asɩ thu.
58011001	Ha pɛ hananɛ dʋɔn tu jɩɩr dɩ gɩrɛ sɩ-n pɛnɩ nũu sa 'lɛr, na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩnakɛ dayɩnana', sɩ sɩ jɩrɔ tue dɩ gɩ hale.
58011002	Ha pɛrɛɛkɛra kɔɔ cʋɛ dɩ kɔ̃tɩna mamara kɔɔ hana i bʋɔ Thãgbara.
58011003	Ha pɛrɛra sɩ jɩ dɩ nʋɔ Thãgba kɔɔ sona dɩ thɩɩ na ƴũ kɔɔ ti, dɩ mɛ̃ gɩrɛ sɩ-n yɩnɩ the gɩrɛraakɛ na dɔnɩ dayɩnana'.
58011004	Ha pɛrɛra Abɛl kɔɔ ji bonɩɛ Thãgbara dɩɩ thʋ̃ bɔr ka a jɔ Kayɛ̃ɛda, dɩ gɛrra a kɔɔ 'lɛr i bʋɔ dɩ tɩɩ sarʋ a do mɔ̃ Thãgbara kɔɔ teenɩ ɔɔ khaarda, dɩ ha pɛrɛrara Abɛlɩda hale gɩrɛ 'lo dɩ ga-n mɩɩ sɩɩ dorakɛ a kɔɔ khire.
58011005	Ha pɛrɛra dɔ nɔɔ Enɔkɩ na kɔɔ khinə sa jʋʋn Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩ tibil na kɔɔ puno a yɩɩ bã, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa kɔɔ gbaanɛɛ a jʋʋnna. Dι Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayι ɔbɔɔkɛ aa kɔɔ jʋʋnnι Thãgbaa dʋɔ pa', ɔɔda kɔɔ dar Thãgba haar.
58011006	Dɩ ado ha pɛrɛ na hala', tibil na puno na da Thãgba haar kpιιraka'; gιdonι ʋrɛɛkɛ n wɔrɔnɛnι Thãgba dɔ a pɛr haar dι Thãgba hale, dι ɔr dʋɔn ʋrɛ n 'laanɛnι khor wιrɛraakɛ n ƴaalɛɛnι.
58011007	Ha pɛrɛra Noe kɔɔ pɛ nũu thιɛnaakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ kpãkpaanaanι sι dι ga do a yι gɛr pa'. A kɔɔ pər garɛ a gbɛbιrɔ bato gɩ taa ɔɔ cɔdara. Dɩ gɛrra a kɔɔ heenna tɩbɩla thɩɩra sor, dɩ a 'lɛr Thãgbara fɩl sarʋʋkɛ n thɛnι ha pɛrɛra.
58011008	Ha pɛrɛra Abιraham ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ wιιnι, a kɔɔ nιrɛ nũu a the jal paarιkɛ a na 'lɛnι na hɩ̃; dι a kɔɔ ther da-n jal sι aa jι ka a na jalna'.
58011009	Ha pɛrɛra a kɔɔ jal too dιιraakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnι ιna haarɛ, dι a toorore kpakpal togʋʋ da-n cɔ kẽkẽ waʋ na Ɩjakι na Jakɔbι, wɛrkɛ dɔnι ʋlfɛ bιɛlιlee hɩ̃hɩ̃sɔra.
58011010	Gιdonι dιιkɛ hananι go kpɛɛrɛ dιι tι a-n pιɛr, kɛ Thãgba donι ʋrɛ kheranι mɔ̃ ga mιnι a dona wa mιmι.
58011011	Ha pɛrɛra Saraa thɛthɛrakɛ 'lini tιιn sι a kɔɔ 'lɛr punone a kɔ̃ bi, gιdonι a hananɛ ha pɛrɛ dι ʋrɛ kɔɔ ʋlfɛnɛnι ʋlfɛrɛɛle, sobɔ tibil a do.
58011012	Gɛr gι tιι bιɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽekɛrakɛ wo 'lenɩ sɛlɛlɛ pɩ, 'lɛ məlle dɩ wɩ jɔr a ho ƴepələ̃be ƴũ, a hona gbalãkothιnιkɛ n hanι lanyɔ̃ nʋɔra, kɛ tibil na punoneni na thera'.
58011013	Ha pɛ hʋɛra wele fɛʋ khiir sι wa 'lɛrakɛ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛna wιna', sι wι yι gɛr ƴɔɔ a 'laa fʋɔr gι, dι wι ture dakha kpakpala ha nɩ dɩ ɩnɩ dona kpãkpara thɩɩraakɛ.
58011014	Wɩrɛ n mɩanɩ thakɛ nɩnanɛ casɩ dɩ wɩ-n ƴaalɛ dɩɩkɛ na dɔnɩ awɩda.
58011015	Ado dɩɩkɛ wɩ kɔɔ thernɩɩda n bor dɩ ga-n too awɩ kpɩɛrɛra, ga dor wa kɔɔ yɩrɛ hʋɛ a na kɛr na biro.
58011016	Sɩ dɩɩkɛ baannɩ dɩphã wɩ-n ƴaal ka, a thɩɛna gaa dɩɩkɛ hanɩ ƴũ gɩ. Gɛr gɩ yicuru na fʋ Thãgba wa-n we nɩ awɩ Thãgba gaaga, gɩdonɩ a gbɛbɩ warɛ dɩɩ.
58011017	Ha pɛrɛra Abɩraham kɔɔ jinə Ɩjakɩ bonɩɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ bɩɩnɩ bɩnɛ a hɩɩn; ɔrkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ a kɔɔ gbaarra ɔɔ Bikũu bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ a kɔɔ jinəna bonɩɛ,
58011018	sɩɩ dorakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ sʋʋraarɛ ɔɔdara ayι: “Ɩjakιra fa 'lɛ məlle wa-n wena afι i.”
58011019	A hananɛ kpιɛrɛ dι Thãgba hananɛ punone a na ιιrnaa khirera, dι a thιɛna gaa gι hor khirerara a ιιr dι bir 'lιɛ.
58011020	Ha pɛrɛra Ɩjakι kɔɔ bɔna Jakɔbι na Ejayʋ mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ na ha warnι ƴɛ kʋʋlɔ.
58011021	Ha pɛrɛra Jakɔbι n kɔɔ khi a bɔna Jojɛfιι bikuunsɔ bιɛlbιɛl a gbuu gbʋʋl a wurõwuro sa fʋɔr Thãgba.
58011022	Ha pɛrɛra Jojɛfιι khi bɔ n thɔɔ dι mιι Ɩjιrayɛl bιsanaa theda a mιɛna wι mɔ̃ wa cʋʋnɩ na ɔɔ khubusɔ.
58011023	Ha pɛrɛra Mʋɩjɩɩ thɩ na ɔɔ nɩ kɔɔ keruu pora yẽther bɔɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ kʋɔnɩ, gɩdonɩ wɩ yɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ bɩsaanna thʋnɩ ɓɔ̃, dɩ maar na kɔɔ fʋ wɩrakɛ fãgadaarɩ jɔfʋra ga.
58011024	Ha pɛrɛra ɔbɔɔkɛ Mʋɩjɩra kɔɔ khɔnɩ pɩ bo ayɩ, wa-n we nɩ Faarɔ̃ɔ bikhɛrɩ bikuuna';
58011025	a ka nar wa-n hʋɔlɛ nar nakha Thãgbaa too sa ka bo sopugo kãkarɩkɛ a na kãkanɩ bɔɔ gbe fɩɩʋ dɩbara.
58011026	A hɩɩnɛ beesire na Kirisiti dɩɩ dʋʋraa thɩ̃ ɓʋ̃ɔ a jɔ Ejipiti lẽle thɩ̃ɛ, gɩdonɩ khorɩkɛ a na 'lɛnɩ gɛr a-n hɩɩn kirkirkir.
58011027	Ha pɛrɛra a kɔɔ the Ejipiti dɩɩra sɩ maar na kɔɔ fʋʋrakɛ fãgadaarɩ nĩkhirə ga, gɩdonɩ a harrɛ kĩkĩkĩ a ho a yɩrɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ dayɩnana'.
58011028	Ha pɛrɛra a kɔɔ cʋʋ Pakɩ a jɛbɩna tɔmɩn dɩ mɛ̃ gbõgolõdaar na tha Ɩjɩrayɛldaraa caca birə ga.
58011029	Ha pɛrɛra Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsana kɔɔ ɩɩr lanyɔ̃ sɩɛ dɩɩ ho pa khɩɩ gɩ, sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ Ejipitidara kɔɔ pɛrnɩ haar ɩnɩ-n cʋɛ oti iner, wɩ kɔɔ khiire nyʋɔnɔ.
58011030	Ha pɛrɛra Jeriko gʋʋsɔ kɔɔ jiiro ɔbɔɔkɛ Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsana kɔɔ fini diiro nyẽbe makonyɔ na pɩ.
58011031	Ha pɛrɛra Rahabɩ khɛ pɔɩ na kɔɔ khi na nũ nʋra ga, gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ teere gɩgɩla na ha bʋɔ.
58011032	Dɩ anye hale 'lo dɩ ma bir na so wo? Gɩdonɩ ma yɩ ƴɩɛ na mɩɩ nɩ Jedeyɔ̃ɔda, na Barakɩɩda, na Sãsɔ̃ɔda, na Jefɩtheeda, na Davɩdɩɩda, na Samʋɛlɩda, na Thãgbaa bobonaada ga.
58011033	Ha pɛrɛ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ wɩ kɔɔ puno fãgadarasɔɔ dɩ, wɩ cʋʋrɛ dakha gɩrɛ saranɩ, wɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr gɩrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛna wɩnɩ, wɩ kɔɔ khaanɛ sidũ'ũ gbuokho,
58011034	wɩ kɔɔ kʋkʋʋlɛ dɔɔ fãga, wɩ forre bajɩna kʋrra, wɩ kɔɔ ther yɔɔrɛra a 'lɛ fãga, wɩ dor kũu khaa kʋʋrra, wɩ weelele sɔrasɩ kpala.
58011035	Khɛr ɩkha bire 'lɛ awɩ tibilsɔɔkɛ ɩrɛnɩ a the khirera. Tibil ɩkhasɔ n kɔɔ 'wãga dɩ wa-n khinə, sa bo fuure wɩ puno wɩ 'lɛ khi ɩɩrɛɛkɛ baannɩ.
58011036	Ɩkhasɔ hire maanɛ na ciile, na jɔrkɔ lir, na khaɩ tʋʋr.
58011037	Wɩ kɔɔ dʋʋrɛ ɩkhasɔ na bokana a kʋʋr, a vaar ɩkhasɔ na thɩr khaadaa, a kʋʋr ɩkhasɔ na bajɩna, bana lʋʋ na bʋ lʋʋ ɩkhasɔ n kɔɔ to dɩ wa-n finə bilili, a 'leena thɩ̃ɛ phuphuphul, wɩ-n kpoo warɛ dɩ wa-n ʋ̃ʋ war.
58011038	Tɩbɩlaalera na teena thɩɩka'. Wɩ-n kpaarɛ bəənnə, na gɔ̃gɔnana, wɩwɩl kanana na bi kpololo wɩ-n kɔɔ cɔ.
58011039	Wele fɛʋʋle wɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr i bʋɔ Thãgbara awɩ ha pɛ hanana, sɩ wa kɔɔ 'lɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛna wɩna'.
58011040	Thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ a ka Thãgba thɩɩn asɩ thɩɩn, dɩ ga do a-n ƴaalɛ gɩ dɔ wɛr bʋɔnɔ a dã thu sɩɩ do ser na halaa ga.
58012001	Gɛr gɩ sɛrɛ dakha mɔ̃ sɩ hananɩ yi tordara dɩ wɩ jɔr tə̃tə̃tə̃ a jɛ kpala sar, dɔ sɩ faa gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔ sarnɩ heendaa na sopugookɛ na-n pʋɔrɛnɩ sɩ dɩɩ barã sa', sɩ sa-n ca na yɩrrɛ kɔlɔ̃kɔɔkɛra phɩnanɩ asɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn,
58012002	sa-n hɩɩnna Jeju kirkirkir, kɛ ha pɛrɛ n thernɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ dakha ʋrɛ n cʋɛnɩ ha pɛrɛ dɩɩ jɩɩ do ha pɛrɛ. Daʋʋkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ thɩɩnaanɩ dɔ nɔɔ dɩ kɔɔ gaar bʋɔ na ha fʋrɛ kʋkʋ thɩrʋra, sɩ aa kɔɔ therna yicuruukɛ gɩ-n hanana', dɩ nɛnɛ̃ a toore Thãgbaa fãga too pa nyɔ̃bɔɔra.
58012003	Na-n jɩɛ kpɩɛrna ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ fʋɔnnɩ haar bo ca olela ɓoɓo sopugodara kɔɔ bʋʋnɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ na vɔa', dɩ nyɛ̃ɛ na khiir ni dakha ga.
58012004	Anɩ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ na sopugo ga jalna nɩ pɩ dɩ tɔmɩn thʋ̃ tha'.
58012005	Nɩ diinəne fɩl dɩɩr thɩmɩɩrɩle ya? Mee bikũu dʋʋrra Thãgba so nar ayɩ: “Ɩ̃ bikuun, na pərə Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wɛbɩra; ado a na naar fɩ, fa-n do haar n kʋɛ fa'.
58012006	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn nanɩ, ɔr a-n wɛbɩ, ʋrɛ a-n wenɩ bikuun ɔr a-n ciil.”
58012007	Anɩ wɛbɩ dɔ nɔɔ dɩɩ teena nɩ to gaarɛ. Thãgba n hɩɩn nɛr mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ ɔɔ bikuunsɔ; gɩdonɩ ʋmɔ̃ɔ bikuun haanle dɩ thɩrɛ na wɛbʋa?
58012008	Ado Thãgba na-n wɛbι nι bikona fɛʋʋ kha ga, ga dor khɛ pɔɩɩ bιsãsɔ nι do, ga do bikũu bɔ nι doa'.
58012009	Dιrakɛ asι thιsɔ kɛ thιιraakɛ n kɔɔ wɛbι sɛr, sι sι-n kɔɔ cʋ wɛr, dι ga ka teena sι wuro jɔ ƴũ Thιrɛra a 'lɛ yirəə?
58012010	Bɔɔ gbe asι thιsɔ kɔɔ wɛbι sι mɔ̃kɛ wι yιɛnι dιι bɔr, sι Thãgba n wɛbι sɛr thɩ̃ɛ n bɔ sar sι puno sι phu mɔ̃kɛ a phuni.
58012011	Sobɔr gι wer, wɛbιrɛ fɛʋ ga-n do daʋ fʋ paara', gbobire gι-n do, sι pιpιι paar ha ιι gι-n do dιι ιna dakha fιlɛɛkɛ saranι wιrɛraakɛ lonanι wɛbιrɛraalera.
58012012	Gɛr gι nι dɔ anι nyɛ̃ɛkɛ ƴʋɔlɛnι n hιl nar, anι nɛkhilikɛ taanɛnι n bir gι sar.
58012013	Nι dɔ anι nɛ na-n gba hʋ telẽe dι mɛ̃ gbãgbarʋʋ nɔ na ɓɔra', sι gι ka gι kpɛɛ.
58012014	Na-n ƴaalɛ ha ie toore na tιbιla fɛʋ na kpιι leere, gιdonι ado kpιι leere na hala', tibil bιɛllakɛ na yι Kɔ̃tιna'.
58012015	Na-n jιɛ dʋ bʋrɛ dι tibil bιɛl na-n 'lee Thãgbaa bɔ ja', thιr nɛ khaa na-n phu dakha a na pɛ nyanyaanɛ anι thɩ̃thιιn gι ho ga mar tibil jɔjʋɔa'.
58012016	Na-n jιɛ dʋ bʋrɛ tibil na-n do bɔdɛl cʋʋdaara', dι dakhabaa gι Ejayʋʋ kha ga, kɛ wi bιɛl dιkor donι nɔɔ dι faarɔ ɔɔ hʋ hana mɔ̃ a donι caca bikuuna'.
58012017	Nι jιrɛ a gι pιrɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ a ƴaalnι a bir a 'lɛ ɔɔ thιι bɔna, a kɔɔ bʋʋrɛ sιrakɛ a kɔɔ ƴaal gɛr na yilẽbe, sι ga do thɩ̃ɛ na punone na debi bã.
58012018	Ga do gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔɔkɛ tibil na punoni na thar nι wɔrɔ̃a', kɛ dɔnι dɔ haara', kɛ hanι kukukulə', dι dabirə ga, dι thãgba jɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι ga,
58012019	dι tutuu ʋʋn ga, dɩ nɔ khena ga, mɔ̃kɛ wɛkɛ kɔɔ nɩɛnɛnɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlnɩ dɩ ɩna-n bir a nɩ gɩrakɛ bã;
58012020	gɩdonɩ wa mar ga thɩmɩɩlera sɔnɩ thaka', gɩ yɩ: “Ado nʋm gɩrakɛ sa thar gɔ̃gʋɔnaale bokana wa dʋʋrnaa a na kʋ.”
58012021	Dι thɩ̃ɛɛlera wι garnι yire n kɔɔ kʋrɛ maar ka, dι Mʋιjι ba sona ayι, maar hor ga tɔ nɛr na kpɛɛ dι ιna-n jẽ.
58012022	Sι ne wer Sιyɔ̃ gɔ̃gʋ̃ɔ nι wɔrɔ̃, kɛ dɔnι Thãgba yidaarι dι, kɛ dɔnι ƴũ Jerujalɛm, ka thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃ hanι,
58012023	a wɔrɔna wιrɛ gbɛbanι kha dι wa-n kãka, kɛ dɔnι Thãgbaa caca bikuunsɔɔ kpa jɛ pa, kɛ awι i kherenι Thãgbaa dʋɔ; nι wɔrɔnɛ dakha kιιldaarιkɛ dɔnι tιbιla fɛʋʋ Thãgba, a wɔrɔna tιι saraakɛ Thãgba cʋʋnι dιphã dι wι bɔr a dã thu,
58012024	a wɔrɔna Jejuukɛ dɔnɩ ƴɛƴɛɛ dɩɩ do nɔɔ dɩ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛ phaa hale, a wɔrɔna tɔmɩ̃ jɛbɩrɛɛkɛ n jɩɛnnɩ khe a ba Abɛlɩda.
58012025	Na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn, na-n bo ʋrɛɛkɛ n mɩana', gɩdonɩ ado wɛkɛ kɔɔ bɔnɩ Thãgbaadaakɛ ʋrɛ kɔɔ hanɩ thɩɩra n mɩɩ wɩnɩ na kɔɔ puno a fuə', mɔ̃ ser na fʋ sɩ na fuu ado sɩ bo ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnɩ ƴũ sɩ da-n mɩɩ.
58012026	Ɔɔ nɔ kɔɔ jɩɩn thɩɩkɛra dabɔɔlera; dɩ nɛnɛ̃ a ʋlfɛrɛ gɩrɛ wo ayɩ, ɩna bire na jẽ thɩɩ babɩɛl wo, sɩ ga do thɩɩ gɩ dɩphã dɩbara ga sɩ na thãgbara ƴũ.
58012027	Dɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ: “Babɩɛl wo” n nɩnanɛ dɩ thɩ̃ tinəne na jɩɩn a na hɛllɔ, sɩɩ do gɩrɛ na dɔnɩ dajenana' gɛr jɩlɛ.
58012028	Gɛr gɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ hanɩ gɩrɛ dɩ sa-n 'lɛ fãga dɩɩkɛ na dɔnɩ datutugonaa ga, dɔ sɩ hana fɔfʋɔr haar sa-n fʋɔrna Thãgba gɩ do fʋɔrɛɛkɛ na daaraanɩ haar, na cʋrɛ nakha maar.
58012029	Gɩdonɩ asɩ Thãgba dor dakha dɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ kʋɛ dɔɔ.
58013001	Na-n yɩra a na na kha mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ omɩna.
58013002	Na-n pərə a na tea kpakpala, gɩdonɩ thalee cʋʋ ʋkhasɔ n kɔɔ teero thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ sɩ wa-n kɔɔ ja'.
58013003	Na-n jɛna wɩrɛ hanɩ khaɩra gɩ ho khaɩdarara ha nɩ ner; na-n jɛna wɩrɛ wɩ-n kpooronɩ gɩdonɩ nɛrɛ dakha tomɩrra nɩ hana.
58013004	Dɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na-n hɩɩn her gɩ do thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hananɩ cʋrɛ, dɩ thɩ̃ bise na-n lõ herraala'. Gιdonι Thãgba na kιιlnanɛ wιrɛ dɔnι bɔdɛl cʋʋdara, na khɛ kpιι ƴaaldara, na kũu kpιι ƴaaldara.
58013005	Anι ιιr para na-n do war laarɛ n ho ga hərə nera', sι nι dɔ ga-n da nar na gιrɛ nι hananι, gιdonι Thãgbaa thɛthɛ sɔ ayι: “A gι dʋ mɔ̃ dʋ mɔ̃, sι ma hana faarɛ na faa fa'; ma sι far dιbara kpιιraka'.”
58013006	Dι gɛr gι sι punone so na tu jιιr ayι: “Kɔ̃tιn dʋɔn ɩ̃ bubul, maar na fʋ mι thιɛna ga; anye tibil na puno na cʋʋ mɩ?”
58013007	Na-n jɛna anɩ thɔthɔɔdaraakɛ kɔɔ mɩa nɩnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ. Nɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ awɩ yi khu pa hanɩ, sɩ na phɛla awɩ ha pɛ.
58013008	Mɔ̃ Jeju Kirisiti hanɩ de, mɛna a ha nĩ na bɔɔ khorr.
58013009	Na-n do dɩɩr kpɩɩsɔ dɩɩdɩɩ n cʋʋ nɩ nɩ lɛ̃ hʋɛra ga, gɩdonɩ gɩ bɔrɛra gɩ do Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sɩ tɩ, sɩ ga-n do dɩko thɩmɩɩr gɩ, kɛ na kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ wɛkɛ ma garnɩ yʋʋ bɔaa ga.
58013010	Sɩ hananɛ bonɩ ji paar, kɛ wɩrɛ n dɔnɩ thɔma kẽkẽ waaraale na hananɩ hʋɛ a na khoro thɩ̃a'.
58013011	Nʋmaakɛ gbõdaar n gbanɩ, ga tɔmɩ̃ a lona pa phuurə a jinə sopugo hɛl bonɩɛ, khuirə wɩ-n thena gɩ dɩ wɩ thii dɩɩ hɩ̃.
58013012	Gɛrra gɩ dɩ Jeju dakha, mɔ̃ a na fʋnɩ sɩ na gba ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ tɔmɩ̃ a phʋɔlna tɩbɩla wɩ phu, kɔɔ gaar bʋɔ dɩ khuirə.
58013013	Gɛr gɩ sɩ thɛ a na jalalaa le khuirə a to beesi ca bɩɛlla na ɔɔda.
58013014	Gɩdonɩ sa hana kɛ thɩɩra dɩɩkɛ na jalanɩ ƴɛrra', sɩ dɩɩkɛ na ɩnanɩ sɩ-n ƴaal.
58013015	Gɛr gɩ sɩ gba khɩɩrɛ gɩ do bonɩ ji thɩ̃ɛ sa-n khɩɩna Thãgba bɔɔ fɛʋ, gɩ do Jeju dɔ nɔɔ, a thɩɛna gaa khɩɩrɛɛkɛ asɩ delẽbi n khɩɩnɩ ɔɔ i gɩ.
58013016	Sɩ na-n diinə bɔ cʋʋrɛ na tibil bullə', gɩdonɩ ga bonɩ ji caale n da Thãgba haar.
58013017	Na-n nɛ anɩ thɔthɔɔdara nũu, nɩ wuro war a jɔ, gɩdonɩ wɛr n bɛra anɩ thu mɔ̃ wɩ donɩ wɩrɛ na mɩanɩ Thãgbara mɔ̃ awɩ thɔ̃ hanɩ. A na cʋʋ mɛ̃, wa-n jɩɛ do awɩ thɔ̃ na daʋ ga do war sɩɩra', gɩdonɩ gele thale na ɩna nar bɔɔ fɩɩʋraka'.
58013018	Nɩ bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba na pɛ sar. Sɩ jɩɛ jɩ dɩ sɩ hananɛ haarɩkɛ na-n heene sɩnɩ sora', mɔ̃ sɩ-n ƴaalnɩ dɩ sa hana fɩl bʋɔ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra.
58013019	Thɩ̃ɛ gɩ dɩ ma-n bɩɛl nɩ na haar fɛʋ nɩ cʋɛ Thãgba n ha mɩ hʋɛ ɩ̃ puno ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa kɔrɔ.
58013020	Dɔ Thãgbaakɛ ha ɩɩ n thernɩ, kɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ Jeju asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ dɔnɩ bana khedaar kɔ̃tɩn khirera, dɩɩ do tɔmɩnɩkɛ n nɛnanɩ nɔ bɩɛl ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ khorrdaara gɩ the,
58013021	n ha nɩ thɩ̃ bɔɩ fɛʋʋkɛ dananɩ nɩ puno na-n cʋʋ ɔɔ tuur, a na-n cʋʋ sar dakha gɩrɛ daaraanɩ, ga-n the Jeju Kirisitira; dɔ ɔr n hɩ̃ i dʋbɩrɛ bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
58013022	Mɩ-n bɩɛl nɛr omɩna dɩ na fʋ haar fɩl dɩɩr thɩmɩɩrraakɛ mɩ khere narnɩ ga donɩ gɩ kpɛra'.
58013023	Nɩ jɛna dɩ wɩ tire Timothe asɩ omi khaɩra a faa. Ado a ɩnɛ kɔrɔ sa pɔr kha a na yɩ nɩ.
58013024	Nɩ fʋɔrɛ anɩ thɔthɔɔdarasɔ fɛʋ na tɩɩ phuusɔ fɛʋ. Ɩtalɩdara fʋɔr nɛr.
58013025	Thãgba na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra. Amɛn.
59001001	Mɛr Jakɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃daar na Jeju Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩnɩda, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a fʋɔrna caar yʋɔr yenyɔɔkɛ bɩ̃bɩlanɛnɩ a ha paar fɛʋ.
59001002	Ɩ̃ omisɔ, bɔ gaar caar dɩɩdɩɩkɛ nɩ-n yɩnɩ, nɩ gba gɩ ga-n do nar da kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ,
59001003	na-n jɩnana, ado anɩ ha pɛ bo jɩɩl ɔbɔɔkɛ nɩ 'lɛnɩ bɩ̃ ber pɩ, ga dor gɩrɛ na hana nɩhɩ ha fʋrɛ;
59001004	dɩ nɩ dɔ ha fʋrɛ n do ɔɔ thɔ̃ gɩ jɩɩ dã, nɩ jɩɩ bɔr nɩ ka nɩ dã, na thʋ̃ thɩɛna ga.
59001005	Dɩ ado tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra 'lee kpɛsɛrɛ, dɔ ntɛ n bɩɛl Thãgbaraakɛ n 'laanɛnɩ na haar sɩ phaanɛ na-n hala', dɩ Thãgba na haarɛ.
59001006	Sɩ a bɩɛlnɛ gɩ na ha pɛrɛ sɩ a na-n baalɔ fɩɩʋraka', gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n baalɔnɩ a hʋrɛ lanyɔ̃ khɔrɔ̃ɔkɛ jɩɛ n benɩ dɩ ga-n phe bababa.
59001007	Tibil ca ole na-n kpɩɛr ɩna 'lɛr dɩkharakɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ pa ga.
59001008	Tibil gɩɩkɛ n ƴeƴerenenɩ, aa-n jɩɩl pa bɩɛla'.
59001009	Dɔ omineekɛ wa-n thernana' na-n kãka ɔɔ ɩɩrra,
59001010	dɩ lẽle dakha na-n kãkanɛ ɔɔ wurrə; lẽle dor ʋrɛ na phɔnɩ na ka hɔ̃ phɩ̃ khaa.
59001011	Wireekɛ n phananɩ na kporre phãphãphã a-n khιrɛ hʋɔn, dɩ phɩ̃ɩ n jɛ dɩɩ do ɔɔ ɓɔ̃ kʋɛrɛ koo; mɛ̃ lẽle na ɔ̃'ɔɔlɔ̃ ɔɔ thɩ̃ cʋʋ pa a na jɛ.
59001012	Gɩ da tibilləəkɛ n fʋɔnnɩ haar fifiləlela, gɩdonr ado a 'lɛ bɩ̃ ber pɩ, a na 'lɛr khor cacadaar dʋʋrra, kɛ dɔnɩ yidaa, kɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ ʋlfɛnɩ ɩna har wɩrɛ n naan nɩnɩ.
59001013	Sɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ tibil n yɩnɩ fifiləle a na-n yɩ, Thãgba n fifiləne na'; gɩdonɩ Thãgba na ha fifilə paar puure n dʋʋraa fifιləla', dɩ ɔɔ thɛthɛrakɛ na-n fifɩlə tibilə'.
59001014	Tibil n 'lɛr fifiləle ɔbɔɔkɛ thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛ n kʋʋnɩ thue dɩɩ fʋʋ a ɩɩrɔ.
59001015	Dɩ ado thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛlera hana pɛmɛr sopugo a-n kɔ̃, dɩ a sopugo kɔ̃ pɩ dɩɩ do khir a kɔ̃.
59001016	Ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ na-n dədəa koe;
59001017	thɩ̃ bɔɩ fɛʋʋkɛ sɩ-n 'lɛnɩ na khaarda ɓɔna fɛʋ ƴũ gɩ the dahɩrɛ Thɩrɛɛ pa, kɛ na dɔnɩ dadebinaa ga, aa-n file mɔ̃ jəəre n filena'.
59001018	Ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ ƴaalla gɩ the dɩ kɔ̃ sɩ dɩɩ do sobɔ thɩmɩɩrra gɩ the, dɩ mɛ̃ ga do sɛr hʋɔn cacadara ɔɔ thɩ̃ tinəsɔraakɛ a tini.
59001019	Gɛr gɩ ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ mι-n nanɩ, dɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl na-n pɛ thɩmɩɩr nũu kɔrɔ, sɩ wa-n phana kɔrɔ a na mɩɩ thɩ̃a', wa-n phana kɔrɔ a na gba nĩkhiə'.
59001020	Gɩdonɩ tibil nĩkhii na-n cʋʋ dasarʋʋkɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ ga-n cʋɛa'
59001021	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ, nɩ dɔna thɩ̃ bise fɛʋ na bɩ̃ kpallɛsɔ fɛʋ a faa, sɩ na tea na hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ sorɩkɛ n direni anɩ bɩnɔ, kɛ hananɩ fãga a na taa nɩ.
59001022	Na-n dɔ Thãgbaa so cʋʋdara, na-n do nũ pɛdara dɩbara gɩ ho dɩbara nɩ-n fɩɩla'.
59001023	Gɩdonɩ ado tibil na pɛ Thãgbaa so nũu sɩ aa-n cʋa', a hʋrɛ tibilikɛ n hɩnɛnɩ ɔɔ ƴɛ hɩɩnʋna dɩ jɩ mɔ̃ a hanɩ.
59001024	A a hɩɩn sɩ na tɔ gbe dɩɩ do a diinəne dapaara mɔ̃ a hanɩ.
59001025	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ ganɩ ɔɔ yi jɔfʋ ɓʋɔna, kɛ dɔnɩ wa do jɔfʋ da-n yɩrrɔ, dɩ ga-n do aa-n pɛ nũu a bir a diinə ga, sɩ a na-n cʋʋ gιrɛ gι-n sonι, wa tibil caale na 'lɛr bɔnanɛ ɔɔ cʋʋrara a-n cʋʋnι.
59001026	Ado tibil yι Thãgba fɔr ha nι, sι aa-n fʋ ɔɔ delẽbi bɔɔbɔa', ɔɔbara a-n fιιl, ntɛɛ Thãgba fʋɔrιle mɔlɔ gι.
59001027	Thãgba fʋɔr bʋɔɔkɛ na hananι dι paar Thãgba Thιrɛɛ ƴɛra ga dʋɔn khilə̃bi hιιnɛ na khikhɛra awι bɔ gaarra, fι fʋna dakha dιbara fa bise na thιιkɛɛ thɩ̃ bisə'.
59002001	Ɩ̃ omisɔ, nɛrkɛ pɛnι haar asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitiraakɛ dɔnι i dʋbιdaar, na-n hana tibil hιιnɛ dιιdιa'.
59002002	Ado tibilikɛ tɔnι dɛ nyɛ̃bi tʋʋ na kẽkẽ ɓʋ̃ɔ, kɛ dɔnɩ lẽledaar lõ anɩ gbɛbɩ pa, dɩ a bɔdaar dakha to ɔɔ kẽkẽ sɛlɛ a lona,
59002003	dɩ ado nɩ hɩɩnɛ ʋrɛ tɔnɩ kẽkẽ ɓʋ̃ɔɔle a sʋʋraa ayɩ: Tɔɔ kɩɛr too pa ɓʋɔnaakɛ lee; sa ka so bɔdaarra: Fer n jɩlɛ liir; agɩbo: Tɔɔ kɩɛr thʋnɔ ɩ̃ nɛ ballɔ.
59002004	Ga do gele n dɔ tibil hɩɩnɛ dɩɩdɩɩ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩnaa? Dɩ ga do kɩɩl gõgolõ nɩ-n kɩɩlaa?
59002005	Ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, nɩ pɛ nũu: Thãgba na kɔɔ phiir wɩrɛ dɔnɩ bɔdara thɩɩraakɛ dɩ wa debi na do lɛ̃lɛ ha pɛdaara na wɩrɛ na lonanɩ Thãgba fãgadaarɩ dɩraakɛ a kɔɔ ʋlfɛnanɩ wɩrɛ n naanɛɛnaa?
59002006	Sɩ ner na-n beesi bɔdaarɩ. Ga do lɛ̃lɛ n hʋɔlɛ nar dɩ wɩ pɛ nar nyɛ̃ kheu a haal nɩ na jalna kɩɩl paarraa?
59002007	Ga do wɛr n kpɛ i ɓʋ̃ɔɔkɛ wɩ ha nɩnaa?
59002008	Ado ger nɩ-n cʋʋrɛ gɩrɛ Thãgba fãgadaar jɔfʋ sonɩ ɔɔ sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Fa-n na afɩ 'walãkha tibil mɔ̃kɛ fɩ-n nanɩ afɩbara”, ga dor nɩ-n cʋʋrɛ bɔɔ.
59002009	Sι ado nι hananɛ tibil hιιnɛ dιιdιι sopugo nι-n cʋʋ, dι jɔfʋ na heen ner sor anι nũ nʋʋrra.
59002010	Gιdonι tibil wo tibilikɛ n hιnɛnɩ jɔfʋ fɛʋ sɩ a a dɩ jɔfʋ bɩɛlla 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ, jɔfʋ fɛʋ a dɩrɔ.
59002011	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ: “Fa-n hana khɛ kpɩɩ ƴaala', fa-n hana kũu kpιι ƴaala'”, ɔrra sɔ dakha wo ayι: “Fa-n kʋ tibilə'.” Dɩ ado fa-n ƴaal khɛ kpɩa', fa-n ƴaal kũu kpɩa', sɩɩ do tibil fɩ kʋ, jɔfʋ kʋɛdaarra fɩ do.
59002012	Mɛ̃ gɩ na-n mɩa thɩmɩa a na cʋɛna thɩ̃ɛ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ donɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ wa do jɔfʋ na kɩɩlnanɩ.
59002013	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ bɔ jɩɩra', ɔɔ kɩɩlɩkɛ a na 'lɛnɩ ga hana bɔ jɩɩr dakha ga, dɩ bɔ jɩɩr n punone kɩɩlʋ.
59002014	Ɩ̃ omisɔ, anyee bɔ ca ga taa tibil da so nayɩ, ɩnɩ hananɛ ha pɛrɛ, sɩ gɩ do thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ na hala'. A na punone na 'lɛ taarɛ na ha pɛ ca ole ya?
59002015	Ado õkona wɛ, a õkhɛna wɛ a 'lee kɩ̃kɩɩn, a 'leena wire fɛʋ dɩkɔ,
59002016	dɩ tibil bɩɛl nɛrɛra so war ayɩ: Nɩ kɔna bɔɔ, a tɔ kɩ̃kɩɩn gɩ kpor nar, a khɔna dakha dɩkɔ a he; sɩ na ha wɩ gɩrɛ teananɩ gɩ bul wa', anyee bɔ ca gele na taa?
59002017	Mɛ̃ gɩ ha na ha pɛrɛ, ado ga hana thɩ̃ cʋʋra', gɩ khire juu.
59002018	Sɩ ʋkha na sor: Fe wer fɛr hana ha pɛrɛ, sɩ mɛrɛ dɩ ɩ̃ hana thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ. Sɩ ma birseere: Dɩ nɛ mar mɔ̃ afɩ ha pɛ fʋnɩ sa hale, sɩ ga hana thɩ̃ cʋʋra'. Sι mɛrɛ ma nιna fɛr na ɩ̃ thɩ̃ cʋʋ mɔ̃ ɩ̃ ha pɛ hanι.
59002019	Fι pɛrɛ haar Thãgba bιɛl haanlaa? Gι bɔrɛ. Kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔ n pɛrɛ mɛ̃ haar wer sι dι wa-n jẽ.
59002020	Sι fɛr də̃bəəlu, fa-n ƴaal fι jι dι ado ha pɛrɛ na-n hana thɩ̃ cʋʋra', ga do bɔ taa ha pɛrɛ gaagaa?
59002021	Thãgba na kɔɔ we asι mama thι kɔ̃tɩ̃ Abιraham tιι sarʋ thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra, dιι do gιrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ gbanι ɔɔ bikuun Ɩjakι a jinə bonιɛ gι thaa?
59002022	Fa yι gaa, ɔɔ ha pɛ na thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ fʋrɛ kha, dι dakha ɔɔ thɩ̃ cʋʋra dor nɔɔ dι ɔɔ ha pɛ thʋ̃ bɔr ka.
59002023	Mɛ̃ gιrɛ kherenenι Thãgbaa sɛbɛra dã oti ayι: “Abιraham kɔɔ pɛr Thãgba haar dιι do gɛr Thãgba hιιn sa wιι tιι sarʋ” na Thãgbaa kuun.
59002024	Na yι gaa, thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛra Thãgba n hɩɩn tibil dɩ do tɩɩ sarʋ, ga do ha pɛrɛra gɩ dɩbara ga.
59002025	Rahabɩ khɛ pɔɩ, ga do ɔr dakha Thãgba hɩɩnʋʋnɛ dɩ do tɩɩ sarʋ gιrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ cʋʋnι, kɛ dɔnι mɔ̃ a teenι thɔ̃thɔna a cʋʋ wι dι wι fuunə hʋ kpιaa?
59002026	Gιdonι mɔ̃ tomιr na-n hananι thueə', dιι do gι khire, mɛ̃ gι ha pɛrɛɛkɛ na-n hananι thɩ̃ cʋʋra', ha pɛ khire gι.
59003001	Ɩ̃ omisɔ, tibil jɔjʋɔ na-n ƴaal ιnι-n dɔ dιιrdara ga, gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sɛr dɩɩrdara na 'lɛr kɩɩlʋ dɩ ga khɩɩr na ka.
59003002	Sɛrɛ fɛʋ sɩ-n dɩrɛ thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔra ka. A tibil na-n dɩ thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛra ga ɔr dɔ tɩɩ bʋɔ ka, a na puno ɔɔ tomɩ na fʋ kĩkĩ.
59003003	A sɩ pɛ gãgʋʋ ther nɔɔ wa-n nɛ sɩ nũu, sɩ-n punone dɩ sɩ ma awɩ tomɩra koo.
59003004	Nɩ yɛ dakha mɔ̃ bato kɔ̃tɩna n hanɩ; gɩ-n kɔ̃tɩnɩnakɛ thale dɩ jɛ kʋkʋʋlʋ n cʋʋ gɩ dɩ ga-n ca, sɩ fɩɩʋ vɩrdaa n ha, kɛ vɩvɩr n vɩrnanɩ dɩ ga-n jal kãkɛ a-n ƴaalnɩ ga-n jala.
59003005	Mɛ̃ dakha delẽbire ha; tomɩ ɓã buu gɩ fɩɩʋ, sɩ a-n punone nɔ fa mɩɩrɛ ka. Nɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ dɔkpõbire n thiini bə̃ kʋkʋʋ tə̃ə.
59003006	Dɩ delẽbire dakha dɔɔ gɩ. Delẽbire hʋrɛ puureekɛ henɩ gɩrɛ thɩɩra; a har asɩ tomɩ ɓãsɔra da-n bise tomɩr koo. Ɔr n ləbire si asɩ yi hanana koo na dɔɔkɛ bu pa dɔɔ n ləbinaanɩ.
59003007	Hɔ̃ nʋ̃ caar ɓibi, na 'lomĩ caarsɔ, na thɩ̃ ƴɩrɛ n puulonenisɔ, na thɩ̃ ƴɩrɛ hanɩ lanyʋɔnna, thɩ̃ɛsɔ gɩɩkɛ tibil na punoni na jo dɩ wɩ 'lire puno wɩrakɛ dɩ wɩ jo.
59003008	Sɩ delẽbire tibil na-n puno dɩ maaraa dɩ joa', thɩ̃ puu gɩ aa ha ma paara', khi kpal haar a hinə koo.
59003009	Ɔrra sɩ-n khɩɩna Kɔ̃tɩn asɩ Thɩ, dɩ ɔrra wo sɩ-n nɩɩrna tɩbɩlaakɛ Thãgba tini dɩ wɩ hʋʋ.
59003010	Nɔ bɩɛllaalera khɩɩrɛ na nɩɩrɛ n the. Ɩ̃ omisɔ ga teena ga-n hana thala'.
59003011	Yɔ bu ka bɩɛlla na-n bure yɔ daa wo a bir a na-n bunə yɔ ƴʋ̃ɔ ya?
59003012	Barʋ punone se thɩn ya ɩ̃ omisɔ? Dɩ 'lʋɔ punone se baar ya? Mɛ̃ gɩ, yɔ bu kaarɩkɛ n bonɩ lanyʋɔn na puno na bu yɔ yɔnana'.
59003013	Ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn hana kpɛsɛrɛ a dona thɩ̃ jɩn? Dɔ ɔɔ fɩl bɔ na ɔɔ thɔ̃ɔkɛ a-n cʋʋnι na hɛlɛlɛ fιlɛ na-n nιna dι tιι kpɛsɛ haa.
59003014	Sι ado nɩ hananɛ gbugi tə̃tə̃tə̃ anι hara na dɩbara na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ, na-n too na məbi khaar a kuur sɔ̃sɔ na pɛ sobɔrra ga.
59003015	Kpɛsɛ ca gele ga do ƴũ gι tha', thιdaa gι, a do tibilikɛ na hananι Thãgbaa Thuəəda, kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ pa gι the.
59003016	Gιdonι kãkɛ gbugi n hanɩ na dɩbara na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ, liir nyanyaanɛ na puu cʋʋ caar fɛʋ n the.
59003017	Sɩ kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ mɔ̃ a-n hanɩnakɛ dʋɔn: Aa-n hana dɩ paara', ha ie haar a do, a-n hananɛ bɩ̃ bʋɔ, ɔɔda na-n khɩɩra', bɔ jɩɩr jʋɔraarɛ, a-n hananɛ dakha bɔ cʋʋrɛ, datelẽ haar n thɛ ɔɔ pa, aa hana bɩnɛ yenyɔa'.
59003018	Wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ gɩrɛ n 'laanɛnɩ ha ɩɩ, ha ɩɩ wɩ-n diirnə, dɩɩ do gɩrɛ gɩ-n senɩ dʋɔn fɩl sarʋ.
59004001	Anye n ɩnana kɩla na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn saagado anɩ thɩ̃ ƴaal kpãkpãa kheekɛra n hərəne nini ga?
59004002	Nɩ-n pɩɛrɛ haar sɩ na yɩ ga; tɩɩ kɔ ha nɩ na yeye, sɩ na puno na 'lɛ thɩ̃ɛ kpɩɩraka'. Nɩ hananɛ kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛ na kɩla sɩ na hana dɩkha dɩ ga do anɩda fɩɩʋraka', gɩdonɩ na-n bɩɛl Thãgba ga.
59004003	Nɩ-n bɩɛlɛ sɩ na-n 'la' gɩdonɩ kpιɛr puu nι-n bιɛlna, nι gba na-n kʋɛ anι thɩ̃ ƴaal kpãkpãa khera.
59004004	Nι hʋrɛ khɛrιkɛ hananι kuun sι da-n ƴaal kũu kpιι. Na jι dιι do a tibil na thιιkɛɛ thɩ̃, gι-n pɛr laarɛ na Thãgba gaa? Tibil wo tibilikɛ n naannι thιιkɛɛ thɩ̃, a-n debire dι do Thãgbaa lãlaardaar.
59004005	Thueekɛ Thãgba tinəni tibil, nι pɛrɛ haar mɔlɔ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ so ayι, a hananɛ gbugi thɩ̃ ƴaalɛ ya?
59004006	Sι Thãgba n 'laarɛ bɔ jιιr dιι jɔr dιι ha mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ sɛbɛ sonι ayι: “Thãgba n bãbaranɛ i ƴaaldara, sι a-n jιrɛ dιbara jodara bʋɔra.”
59004007	Dι gɛr gι na-n jɔ anιbara Thãgbara, nι pιɛrɛ Satã kĩkĩ a fuu saa faa nι.
59004008	Na-n wɔrɔnɛ Thãgba a na wɔrɔ̃ nɛr. Nɛr sopugodara, na-n hulo nyɛ̃ɛ, nι dɔ anι ha na-n phu nɛrkɛ n ƴeƴerenenι.
59004009	Nι yɛ mɔ̃ nι donι bɔ kʋ tɩbɩla; na-n bɛ dɩ na-n khɩa. Nɩ dɔ anɩ mãthɩ̃ n debi gɩ do benɩɛ, anɩ da n debi gɩ do gbobire.
59004010	Na-n jɔ dɩbara Kɔ̃tɩnɩ ƴɛra dɩ ɔr na ɩrɛ nɩ.
59004011	Omɩna na-n mɩɩ thɩmɩɩ puunə na pɛ khasɔa'. Ʋrɛ mɩanɩ dapuu ɔɔ omina, agɩbo dɩ 'laa da-n yɩ ɔɔ omiida, jɔfʋ a mɩɩrɔ puure da-n kɩɩlna gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ. Dɩ a fa kɩɩlna gɩrɛ jɔfʋ sonɩ, ga do jɔfʋ hɩ̃hɩn ha fa', sɩ kɩɩldaar ha fɩ.
59004012	Bɩɛl dɩbara dʋɔn jɔfʋ 'laadaar na kɩɩldaar; ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ na punoneni na cʋʋ tibil da 'lɛ taarɛ, agɩbo a bu. Sɩ fɛrɛ, amɛ fɛrkɛ do dɩ fɩ 'laa na yɩ afɩ 'walãkha tibilida.
59004013	Dɩ nɛnɛ̃, nɛrkɛ n sɔnɩ dɩ nɩ yɩ: Nĩ agɩbo cʋɔ sa jaal dɩ ʋrɛra, na too yɛ bɩɛl sɩ ƴabɩ sa-n 'lɛ mũsumo,
59004014	sɩ na jɩ mɔ̃ anɩ yi na hanɩ cʋɔa'. Anye anɩ yi do? Ɩsiirikɛ n bananɩ bɔɔ gbe fɩɩʋ sɩ dɩɩ kur nɩ do.
59004015	Nɩ teenanɛ nɩ ka na sɔ: A Kɔ̃tɩn tu dɩ sɩ hana yire, sa cʋʋrɛ gekɛ na gekɛ.
59004016	Sɩ nɛnɛ̃ na-n ƴaal ire kpãkpalã ga, dɩ na-n sona kuune. I ƴaal caar thakɛ puurore ka.
59004017	Mɛ̃ gɩ ʋrɛ jɛnɩ thɩ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛ sɩ aa-n cʋa', sopugo a-n cʋʋ.
59005001	Dɩ nɛnɛ̃, nɛr lɛ̃lɛ, nɩ pɛ nũu, na-n khɩa a na bɛna lɩɛrɛra puureraakɛ na dana nɩnɩ.
59005002	Anɩ lẽle thɩ̃ n hɩrɛ dɩ ophɛphɛlɛɛ n khor anɩ kẽkẽsɔ.
59005003	Anɩ dɛ na anɩ war dɩrɛ dʋʋn, dɩ awɩ do dɩɩle ɩɩrɛ dɩ ga-n pɛ nar sor, dɩ gɛr na kʋɛa anɩ tomɩ mɔ̃ dɔɔ n hɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ. Pɩpɩɩ bɔɔ gɩ, sɩ nɩ khɩɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ a thɩɩn.
59005004	Nɩ hɩnɛ thɔ̃daraakɛ kɔɔ khanɩ anɩ jʋ sɩ nɩ tɔ̃ wɩ lɩmɩnɛ n hulene, dɩ jʋ khaa hulẽbirə jʋʋnɛ a lõ Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ fãga koo hɩ̃daarɩ nũ kaar.
59005005	Nɩ hananɛ nũfe thɩ̃ɛ kɛ thɩɩra a too kãkarra; nι hire phi a khɔ̃, sιι do kʋkʋ togʋʋ nι too.
59005006	Nι kɔɔ heene tιɩ sarʋ sor a kʋ, sɩ aa kɔɔ so thɩ̃a'.
59005007	Na-n fɔ haar omɩna phaphapharakɛ Kɔ̃tɩn na bire na ɩ̃. Nɩ hɩnɛ kokol n fʋrɛ haar sɩ da-n pɩɛr phaphapha lɩɛra n haa thĩ bʋɔ. A-n fʋ garɛ haar waa dɩ thãgba khaa na pɩpɩɩ thãgba n dana.
59005008	Nɛrɛ dakha na-n fɔ haar ɔmɛ̃ a jɩlɛ kɩbɩ, gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ ɩ̃ bɔ wɔrɔnɛ.
59005009	Na-n hũhuun na pɛ khasɔa' omɩna, dɩ mɛ̃ na 'lɛ kɩɩlʋa'. Nɩ hɩnɛ kɩɩldaar har lõfonɔɔ a jɩɩl.
59005010	Ɩ̃ omisɔ, nɩ gba Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔkɛ kɔɔ mɩanɩ thɩ̃ɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ irəə bɔ gaar na awɩ ha fʋ, gɩ do nar thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ.
59005011	Nɩ hɩnɛ, sɩ-n sor dɩ sɩ yɩ: Gɩ da wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ gaarɛnɩ bʋɔ na ha fʋrɛ. Nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛrɛ mɔ̃ Jɔbɩ kɔɔ fʋnɩ haar, dɩ nɩ jɩrɛ dakha gɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩn kɔɔ cʋʋraanɩ pɩpɩɩ paar, gɩdonɩ bɔ fʋdaar Kɔ̃tɩn do na bɔ jɩdaar.
59005012	Thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩɩnakɛ ɩ̃ omisɔ dʋɔn, na-n ʋlfɛna thãgbara ƴũ dι thιɩkɛ ga; na-n ʋlfɛna dιkhaa thɩ̃ kpιιraka', sι nι dɔ anι “ɔɔ” n do “ɔɔ”, anι “ooho” n do “ooho”, dι mɛ̃ na 'lɛ kιιlʋa'.
59005013	Tibil ʋkha har anι thɩ̃thιιn da-n gaar bʋɔ ya? Ntɛ na-n bιɛlnɛ Thãgba. Tibil ʋkha hale dι daʋ fʋʋ ya? Ntɛ na-n khιna Thãgba nιɛ.
59005014	Tibil ʋkha har anι thɩ̃thιιn dι ga-n khʋʋ ya? Dɔ ntɛ n we we gbɛbιdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ dι wa bιɛl Thãgba na pιɛraa wι pɛnanaa niin na Kɔ̃tιnι i.
59005015	Ha pɛ bιɛlɛ na taarɛ khodaar dɔɔ, dι Kɔ̃tιn na cʋgʋʋrɛ dι na ιιr, dι ado a cʋʋrɛ sopugo Thãgba na faarɛ na haa.
59005016	Gɛr gι na-n cana kha sopugosɔ, sa bιɛlnɛ Thãgba na pɛ khasɔ, mɛ̃ khoo na kpɛɛ nar. Tιι sarʋʋ Thãgba bɩɛl hananɛ fãga ka dɩɩ cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ.
59005017	Tibil Elι do dakha mɔ̃kɛ sι hanι, sι a kɔɔ bιɛlɛ Thãgba na yιrrɛ ƴɛrr thãgba nyʋɔn na-n ɩ̃a', dι thãgba na kɔɔ ɩ̃ ger dιɩ cʋʋna yɛna yẽther na pora maadõa'.
59005018	Sɩ agɩpɩ a bire bɩɛl Thãgba dɩ thãgbara ƴũ 'laa nyʋɔn dɩphã dɩ thɩɩ bir phu thɩ̃ɛ.
59005019	Ɩ̃ omisɔ, ado tibil ha anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn a lɛ̃ sa faa sobɔr dɩ tɩɩ kpɩɩ bir kpaa a pɛ hʋɛra,
59005020	nɩ jɛna dɩ ntɛɛle na kpanɩ sopugodaar dɔɔle ɔɔ bu pa a na birnə, tibil a taa khirrə, dɩ ga dor sopugo jɔjʋɔ thero.
60001001	Mɛr Pɩɛrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔn thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha nɛrɛɛkɛ Thãgba phiirni, kɛ bɩ̃bɩlanɛnɩ gɩrɛ a do kpakpala Pɔ̃, na Galasɩ, na Kapadɔsɩ, na Ajɩ, na Bitini.
60001002	Thãgba Thɩrɛ kɔɔ phire ni dɩɩ do ɔɔ thɩ̃ mãa jιra gι ɩhe, Thu Phuu n lee nɩ kpɩɩ, na-n nι Jeju Kirisiti nũu, ɔɔ tɔmɩ̃ dakha na-n jɛbɩ nar. Thãgba na-n jɛ nɩ bʋɔra jɔɔ, a na-n hana nɩ dakha ha ɩɩ jɔɔ.
60001003	Thãgba asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii Thɩ hɩna khɩɩrɛ, ɔɔ bɔ dona kɔ̃tɩnaakɛ a bironi kɔ̃ sɩ wo dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisitii khi ɩɩrra gɩ the, dɩ sa hana nũ pɛ yire,
60001004	dɩ sa 'lɛ dakha thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na punoneni na kʋɛa', ga puno dakha na bisə', bɔɔkɛ gɩ bɔrnɩ ga puno wo a na deba', dɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ gɩ thɩɩn anɩ thɩɩn,
60001005	nɛrɛɛkɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar dɩ Thãgba na-n bɛr nɩ na ɔɔ fãga nɩ puno nɩ 'lɛ taarɛɛkɛ na yɩranɩ dɩphã pɩpɩɩ bɔɔ.
60001006	Dɩ nɩ hana garɛ kãkar sɩrakɛ gɩ teenanɛ bɔɔ gbe nɩ yɛ bɔ gaar caar dɩɩdɩɩkɛ n hana nɩnɩ gbobire,
60001007	gɩ mɩɛ anɩ ha pɛ gɩ hɩɩn, kɛ ɔɔ the nɔ khɩɩrnɩ a jɔ dɛɛkɛ n kʋɛanɩ, kɛ wɩ-n gbanɩ dɔɔ dɩ wɩ mɩɛna hɩɩn, thale anɩ ha pɛ na hana khɩɩrɛ, a na do i dʋbɩ thɩ̃ɛ, na cʋ thɩ̃ɛ bɔɔraakɛ Jeju Kirisiti na-n mɩ.
