60001008	Nɩ-n naarɛ sɩrakɛ na kɔɔ yɩa', na yɩɩnɩ gɩra', sɩ nɩ pɩɛrɛ haar, dɩ daʋʋkɛ na hanɩ mɩɛrɛra ga a kɔ̃tɩ̃ dakha ka n fʋ nɛr;
60001009	gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ na 'lɛnɩ anɩ ha pɛra pɩpɩɩ paar dʋɔn anɩ thɛthɛɛ taa.
60001010	Thãgbaa bobonaakɛ kɔɔ mɩanɩ bɔ jɩɩrɩdaakɛ Thãgba na jɩ nɩnɩ, kɔɔ ƴaalɛ ka a 'lo wɩ jɩ mɔ̃ taarɛɛdaalera hanɩ.
60001011	Kirisitii Thuukɛ hanɩ awɩ bɩnɔ kɔɔ mãa mɩɩrɛ Kirisitii bɔ gaarda na i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ na kpa garnɩ, a mɩɩ wɛr dɩ wa-n 'lo wɩ jɩ bɔ ca dɔɔkɛ gelela na danɩ na mɔ̃ ga hanɩ.
60001012	Thãgba kɔɔ nɩ warɛ dɩ ga do wɛr na 'lɛ ga thɩ̃ɩlera wɩ-n mɩɩna', sɩ anɩda gɩ. Dɩ nɛnɛ̃, wɩrɛ n mɩanɩ tutugo bʋɔ na Thu Phuu fãgaakɛ thɛnɩ ƴũ kɔɔ mɩa nɩ ga thɩ̃ɩle. Dɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ yɛrɛrakɛ n ƴaalɛ wɩ kpu wa-n hɩɩn ga thɩ̃ɩlera.
60001013	Gɛr gɩ nɩ fɔ dɩbara anɩ kpɩɛrra, a na jʋrɛna, a na pɩɛrna bɔɔbɔɔ bɔ jɩ khaardaakɛ na 'lɛnɩ bɔɔraakɛ Jeju Kirisiti na ɩnɩ.
60001014	Mɔ̃kɛ nũ nɩdara n hanɩ, nɩ hana ɔmɛ̃. Na-n bir na hana thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛkɛ n kɔɔ kɔ nɩnɩ thuee fɩl, mɔ̃kɛ nɩ kɔɔ hana gɩnɩ mamara bɔɔraakɛ nɩ kɔɔ donɩ yʋ 'leedara ga.
60001015	Sɩ mɔ̃kɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ wɛ nɩnɩ donɩ Tɩɩ phuu, nɛrɛ dakha nɩ deba a dɔ tɩɩ phuusɔ anɩ fɩlla fɛʋ.
60001016	Gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Nɩ pho gɩdonɩ mɛrɛ Tɩɩ phuu ha mɩ.”
60001017	Ado nɩ-n wer ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n hɩnɛnɩ tɩbɩla dɩɩdɩa' Thɩrɛ, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ na kɩlɛnanɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl mɔ̃ awɩ thɔ̃ hanɩ, a nɩ jɩ na-n jɩɛ ɩɩr na maar anɩ yi hanana kɛ thɩɩra.
60001018	Gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do, ga do thɩ̃ kʋɛnaakɛ dɔnɩ war na dɛ Thãgba kɔɔ birsena nɩ anɩ thɩthɩsɔɔ də̃bəəl fɩllaakɛ nɩ hanana',
60001019	sɩ Kirisitii tɔmɩ̃ɩkɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ kʋkʋʋ tə̃ə gɩ, mɔ̃kɛ a donɩ bana biikɛ na hananɩ taana', aa hana dakha jiinə'.
60001020	Thãgba kɔɔ mãa phiirəə kɛkɛkɛ sɩ thɩɩkɛ na fʋ tir pa', sɩ pɩpɩɩ bɔɔkɛ a gbaarɛ nɩna dɩphã dɩɩ do anɩda dɔ nɔɔ.
60001021	Ɔr dɔ nɔɔ nɩ pɛrɔnɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba haar, kɛ kɔɔ cʋgɛɛnɩ dɩ ɩɩr a the khirera, a cʋʋnaa dakha dɩ 'lɛ i dʋbɩrɛ, dɩ mɛ̃ anɩ ha pɛ na anɩ nũ pɛ na ha Thãgbara.
60001022	Anɩ nũukɛ nι-n nιnι sobɔr, gι cʋʋ nɛr dι nι phu na-n jιι na anι omisɔɔkɛ nι donanι kha ha pɛdara na naʋʋkɛ huloneni; na-n jιɛ na kha bɩɛlbɩɛl sobɔr na haar fɛʋ,
60001023	nɛrkɛ Thãgba birni kɔ̃ kɔ̃ phaa sɩ ga do thɩ̃ diir kʋɛsʋ kɔna na', sɩ thɩ̃ diireekɛ na dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa gaa gɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩkɛ hananɩ yire, a dona dakha khorrdaa.
60001024	Gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Tibil hʋrɛ hʋɔn, dɩ ɔɔ ɓɔ̃ ɓibi ho hɔ̃ phɩ̃ɩ. Hʋɔn n khɩrɛ dɩ phɩ̃ɩ n jɛ,
60001025	sɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ thɩmɩɩ khorr gɩ ha.” Dɩ ga thɩmɩɩlera dɔ tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ kɔɔ mɩa nɩnɩ.
60002001	Gɛr gɩ nɩ dɔna bɩ̃ kpallɛ fɛʋ a faa, na fɩɩlɛ fɛʋ, na bɩnɛ yenyɔ fɩlɛ, na gbugi, na tɩɩ kuere ɓibi;
60002002	sɩ na-n ƴaalɛ na gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛ ilẽ bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ mɔ̃ bibɔrɔsɔ n ƴaalnɩ ɩlɛ̃, gɛr na khɔnɔ na dana taarɛ,
60002003	gɩdonɩ “nɩ jɩrɛ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ bɔɔkɛ a bɔrnɩ.”
60002004	Na-n wɔrɔnɛ ɔr thɛthɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ boka yireekɛ tɩbɩla kɔɔ bonɩ, sɩɩ do thɩ̃ɛ a do waa gel Thãgbara dɩ phiiruu.
60002005	Dɩ nɛrɛ dakha mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ boka ye, nɩ dɔ Thãgba n gba nɩ a na-n mɩna cʋɔrɩkɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ Thuuda, nɩ doro bonɩ jida phuusɔ na-n ji bonɩɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ Thudaa, kɛ n danɩ Thãgba haar, gɩ do Jeju Kirisiti dɔ nɔɔ.
60002006	Gɩdonɩ gɩ kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayɩ: “Hɩnɛ, mɩ thɩɩnɛ Sɩyɔna go tɩ bokaar, kɛ dɔ marnɩ thɩ̃ɛ waa gel dɩ ɩ̃ phiir. Dɩ ʋrɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar ɔrra, ga ɩ̃ kpɩɩrakɛ a na dʋʋraa yicuruə'.”
60002007	Nɛrkɛ wer pɩɛrnɩ haar, a do narɛ daɓʋ̃ɔ ka, sɩ ado wɩrɛraakɛ na-n pɩɛrnɩ haara gɩ, Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “Bokaarɩkɛ cɔ mɛ kɔɔ bonɩ a do, sɩɩ do ɔr deba a do go tɩ bokaar.”
60002008	Wo: “Nɛ bara bokaar gɩ a dona nɛ bara gbãgbaan.” Wɩ-n berore nɔɔ gɩdonɩ wɩ nʋʋrɛ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩra nũu dɩ ga thɩɩn wɩ kɔɔ thɩɩn wɩrakɛ.
60002009	Sɩ ne wer, nɛr dɔ caarɩkɛ Thãgba phiirni, a dona Fãgadaarɩ bonɩ jidara, nɩ dor ɔɔ tibilsɔɔkɛ phonɩ, na ɔɔ tookɛ a hɩnɩ, gɩ do nɔɔ na-n mɩɩ ɔɔ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ cʋʋ, ɔrkɛ wɛ nɩnɩ dɩ nɩ the dabirəra a lõ ɔɔ nɔ kpaa dahɩrɛra.
60002010	Nɛrkɛ mamara na kɔɔ dɔnɩ ɔɔ toa', nɩ dor nɛnɛ̃ Thãgbaa too; nɛrɛɛkɛ na-n kɔɔ yɛnɩ bɔ jɩɩra', sɩ nɛnɛ̃ Thãgba jɩ nɛr bʋɔra.
60002011	Nɛrkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, nɩ jɛna kpakpala ha nɩ dɩ nɩ dona kpãkpara, gɛr gɩ mɩ-n kpãkpãa narɛ nɩ faa thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛkɛ n kɔ nɩnɩ thue, kɛ n kɛ̃kɛrɛnanɩ thudaa.
60002012	Na-n hana fɩl bʋɔ thɩldaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ thɩ̃ dooraakɛ wɩ-n kue nini dɩɩ ho puu cʋʋdara ha nɩ, wa ƴɩrɛ anɩ thɔ̃ bɔ wa-n khɩɩ Thãgba wireekɛ a na birni na kher nɩ.
60002013	Kɔ̃tɩn dɔ kɩrʋ, gɛr gɩ nɩ jɔ dɩbara ƴɛ kʋlasɔraakɛ fɛʋ tɩbɩla pɛrnɩ, a gobanɛrɩkɛ dɔnɩ yʋʋ gɩ,
60002014	ado fãgadara wɛɛkɛ a pɛrnɩ wa-n heene puu cʋʋdara sor sɩ na khɩa bɔ cʋʋdara;
60002015	gɩdonɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ dʋɔn na-n hana fɩl bʋɔ ga-n khaan dəbələəkɛ na-n jɛnɩ gɩrɛ wɩ-n mɩɩna' nʋɔ.
60002016	Na-n ɩrɛ mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ waɩa, sɩ na-n gba wa dʋʋrɩle a phiro sɩ na cʋʋ gɩrɛ puuronə', sɩ nɩ ka na ɩrɛ mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃dara.
60002017	Na-n cɔ tɩbɩla fɛʋ; na-n na omɩna; na-n ma Thãgba; na-n cɔ fãgadaar.
60002018	Thɔ̃dara na-n jɔ anɩbara anɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔra na maar, ga do kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɔɩra na hɛlɛlɛ fɩldarara dɩbara ga, sɩrakɛ na wɩrɛraakɛ awɩda khɩɩrnɩ.
60002019	Ha fʋʋr bɔ gaarɛraakɛ tibil n yɩnɩ sɩ ga-n do ɔɔ pa dɩɩ tha', sɩɩ do Thãgba a-n nana, gɛr n da Thãgba haar.
60002020	Gɩdonɩ anyee bɔ ca na yɩrɔ ado nɩ cʋʋ sopugo dɩ bɔ gaarɛ ɩ̃ a thʋ nɩ? Sɩ ado nɩ ka na cʋʋ bɔɔ dι ga ιna nar bɔ gaarɛ dι nι fʋrɔ haar, gɛr n da Thãgba haar.
60002021	Gιdonι gelela Thãgba ka we nar, gιdonι Kirisitii thɛthɛ dakha kɔɔ gaarɛ bʋɔ anι sora a nι nar fιlɛɛkɛ na phɛlnι gι do nɔɔ na-n 'loro ɔɔ nɛkara.
60002022	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ na kɔɔ cʋɛnι sopugoə', dι fιιlɛ dakha na kɔɔ the ɔɔ nɔa'.
60002023	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ wι-n kɔɔ nιιrnι sι aa-n bir dι nιιra', a-n kɔɔ gaarnι bʋɔ sι aa kɔɔ so tibilə', sι a kɔɔ faa gɛr a ha ʋrɛ n kιlɛnι kιιl sarʋ.
60002024	Ɔr thɛthɛ dɔ ʋrɛ kɔɔ heenenι asι sopugosɔ ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ tomιra thιrʋra, gι do nɔɔ gι do nι khire sopugo cʋʋrɛra sa hana yire dιι do fιl sardaa. Ɔɔ kho sɛɛkɛ a 'lɛnι dɔ asι kho kpɛɛda.
60002025	Gιdonι nι kɔɔ hor banaakɛ bureni, sι nɛnɛ̃kɛ nι kɛrrɛ bir khekheraakɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ n bɛranι anι thu.
60003001	Mɛ̃ gι ha dakha na nɛr khɛra, na-n jɔ anιbara anι kora, gι do nɔɔ a ιkhasɔ halerakɛ a na nι Thãgbaa thιmɩɩ nũə', sɩ fɩlɛɛkɛ awɩ khɛr hananɩ ga cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wa pɛr haar, sɩ ga dorakɛ khɛr mɩa thɩ̃a';
60003002	sɩ gɩdonɩ wɩ-n yɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ hananɩ fɩl phuu na cʋʋr.
60003003	Na-n barana yʋ lɩɩr, na dɛ thɩ̃ tʋʋr, na kẽkẽ ɓɔ̃ tʋʋr mɔ̃ na bɔrnɩ hɩɩnɛna ga,
60003004	sɩ nɩ dɔ anɩ biir cʋʋ n do hadaa, kɛ dɔnɩ hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ, a ha jɔjɔjɔl ga do dakʋɛnaa ga, gɩdonɩ gɛr dɔ thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra.
60003005	Mɛ̃ khɛ bɔɩɩkɛ mamara n kɔɔ pɛnɩ Thãgba nũu n kɔɔ gbɛbɩ awɩ biir, mɔ̃ wɩ-n jonɩ dɩbara awɩ kora.
60003006	Thale Sara kɔɔ ha. A kɔɔ nɩrɛ Abɩraham nũu a thʋ̃ da-n wɩɩ kɔ̃tɩn, dɩ ɔɔ bikhɛrsɔ nɩ debi do gɩrɛ ado nɩ-n cʋʋrɛ bɔɔ, ado dakha thɩ̃ bιɛl na-n cʋʋ nɩ dɩ maar na-n fʋ na'.
60003007	Mɛ̃ gɩ dakha na nɛr kona, na-n jɩɛ too kha bɔɔbɔɔ na anɩ khɛr mɔ̃ a donɩ tibilikɛ yɔɔnɩ a jɔ nɩ, na-n cʋɔnɛɛ mɔ̃kɛ nɩ bulni kha khaardaakɛ dɔnɩ yireekɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbara, dɩ mɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛ na bãbarã anɩ Thãgba bɩɛla'.
60003008	Ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ kpa pa dʋɔn: Na-n hana kpɩɛrnɔ bɩɛl, na-n hana pəpər haar, nɩ dɔ omi naar, na bɔ jɩɩr, na dɩbara jor n hi ni haarra.
60003009	Na-n gba puure a lɩmɩ puurə'; a tibil nɩɩr nɩ na-n bir nɩɩrʋa', sɩ nɩ ka na bɔnaa, gɩdonɩ gɛr Thãgba we nar dɩ mɛ̃ na 'lɛ dakha bɔnanɛ.
60003010	Dɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “Ado tibil hale a na yi hananɛ, a ƴaal dakha wi bʋɔ na-n phana nar, dɔ ntɛ n fʋ ɔɔ delẽbi thɩmɩɩ puu mɩɩrɛra, na ɔɔ nɔfa fɩɩlɛla.
60003011	Dɔ a hʋnɔna puure, sɩ a na-n cʋʋ bɔɔ. Dɔ ha ii ƴaalɛ n do ɔɔda a na-n gbuuro yʋʋ.
60003012	Gιdonι Kɔ̃tιn n gar ɔɔ yi tιι sarara, dι a-n pɛr dakha awι bιɛl nũu, sι Kɔ̃tɩn n fire khiru di pɛ wɩrɛraakɛ n cʋɛnɩ puure.”
60003013	Amɛ na hʋɔlɛ nar ado na cʋʋ thɩ̃ bʋɔɔkɛ n kɔ nɩnɩ thue?
60003014	Adorakɛ na gaar bʋɔ gɩrɛraakɛ saranɩ, sɩ bɔnadaa gɩ do nar. Na-n ma gɩrɛɛkɛ tɩbɩla n mana'; na-n do haar na-n jẽ nɩ fɩɩʋraka'.
60003015	Sɩ na-n cɔ Kirisiti Kɔ̃tɩ̃ cʋʋr le anɩ hara. Nɩ tɔɔ ga too a na nɛna tibilikɛ n bulene nini kɩrʋ nũ pɛrɛraakɛra nɩ hananɩ, sɩ na-n cʋɛ na hɛlɛlɛ fɩlɛ na maar.
60003016	Na-n hanana dakha kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ na heene nɩnɩ sora', dɩ thɩ̃ dooraakɛ wɩ-n kue nini dɩɩ ho puu cʋʋdara ha nɩ, anɩ fɩl bɔɔkɛ nɩ hananɩ Kirisitira na pɛ warɛ yicuru.
60003017	Gaarɛ thɩ̃ bɔ cʋʋrɛra, ado gɛr n da Thãgba haar, gɩ baar gaarɛ puu cʋʋrɛra.
60003018	Gɩdonɩ Kirisiti dakha kɔɔ khire asɩ sopugora babɩɛl, ɔrkɛ saranɩ khe sɛrɛraakɛ na sarana', dɩ a na kpa sɩ na ha Thãgba. Wɩ kɔɔ kʋrɛ ɔɔ tomɩ wer, sɩ Thue pallɛ ɩɩr na yire.
60003019	Thueelera a jalna a mɩɩ thuesɔɔkɛ hanɩ khaɩra mɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ hanɩ,
60003020	kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ kɔɔ nʋrɛnɩ nũu mamara bɔɔraakɛ Thãgba fʋnɩ haar ƴɛrr Noee bato cʋʋ bɔ, kɛ tɩbɩla fɩɩʋ kɔɔ lʋʋnnɩ, a thɩɛna gaa tɩbɩla makõther wɛ, a kɔɔ taa nyʋɔnna.
60003021	Gɛr n hʋɔn kha na yɔ kpɛɛrɛɛkɛ n taa nɩnɩ nɛnɛ̃, dɩɩ do Jeju Kirisitii khi ɩɩrra gɩ the, dɩ yɔ kpɛɛrɛɛle ga do tomɩ jiin yɔ hʋr ga, sɩɩ do kpɩɛr tir gɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, mɔ̃ sa hananɩ kpɩɛrnɔɔkɛ na heene sɩnɩ sora'.
60003022	Jeju Kirisitira kɔɔ jʋʋnɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ a too Thãgbaa nyɔ̃bɔra, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ punoneni thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ, na fãgadarasɔ, na punodara dɩ wɩ jʋʋraa.
60004001	Gɛr gɩ gɩdonɩ Kirisiti kɔɔ gaarɛ bʋɔ tomɩrra, nɛrɛ dakha nɩ hana ga kpɩɛr ca, gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ gaarɛnɩ bʋɔ tomɩrra a-n sɩrɔrɛ sopugo cʋʋrɛ.
60004002	Thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛkɛ n kɔnɩ tibil thue ga-n do gɛr dɔ ɔɔ yi hana bã, sɩ mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba n ƴaalnɩ a-n hana fɩlɛ ɔɔ yirəəkɛ sɩɛraanɩ kɛkɛ thɩɩra.
60004003	Gɩdonɩ bɔɔkɛ kɔɔ kanɩ gɩ thʋnɛ dã mɛ̃ mɔ̃ nɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ n kɔɔ danɩ thɩldara haar dɩ wa-n cʋʋ. Nɩ kɔɔ faarɛ dɩbara dakhaba cʋʋrɛra, na thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛlaakɛ n kɔ nɩnɩ thue, na ta laarɛra, na gbõgolõ dɩko khorra, na ta yɔ kpãkpaanɛna, na thɩl kpal dɩɩrsɔra.
60004004	Dɩ wɩ yɩɛnɩ dɩɩ kpal war mɔ̃ na-n tuni na-n kpaarɛ kha na wɛr dakhaba thɩ̃ cʋʋ jɔjʋɔraalera bã wɩ-n kue ner;
60004005	sɩ wa mɩɩrɛ awɩda na ha ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnɩ ga too sɩ a na-n kɩɩlna yidara na khe.
60004006	Gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ dakha dɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ wɩrɛraakɛ kɔɔ khenɩ, dɩ ga dor mɔ̃ awɩ tomɩ 'lɛnɩ kɩɩlʋ mɔ̃ wɩ donɩ tibil, awɩ thu na hananɛ yire mɔ̃ Thãgba hana gɩnɩ.
60004007	Thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋ khu pa wɔrɔnɛ, gɛr gɩ nɩ fɔ dɩbara, a na jʋrɛna, a na bɩɛlna Thãgba.
60004008	Sɩ gɩrɛ jɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dʋɔn na-n jɩɛ na kha bɔɔbɔɔ, gɩdonɩ naʋ n thire sopugo jɔjʋɔra.
60004009	Na-n tea kha kpakpaalɛ sɩ hũhuune na-n hala'.
60004010	Mɔ̃ nɩ donɩ wɩrɛ 'lɛnɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ khaardasɔ dɩɩdɩɩ dɩ na-n dona thɔmaakɛ bʋɔnɔnɩ, dɔ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl n gba khaardaakɛra nɩ 'lɛnɩ na-n bulnə ɩkhasɔ.
60004011	Dɩ a tibil 'lɛ punone thɩmɩɩ mɩɩrɛra, dɔ a na-n mɩɩ thɩmɩaakɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa nɔɔ; dɩ a tibil 'lɛ punone thɔ̃ dʋʋrra, a na-n dɔ na Thãgbaa fãgaakɛ a haanɩ; dɩ mɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋra Thãgba na 'lɛr khɩɩrɛ, gɩ do Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the, kɛ hɩnanɩ i dʋbɩrɛ na fãga bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
60004012	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, na-n do gɩ kpal nar gɩ ho nar thɩ̃ phaa, dɔɔraakɛ nɩ hanɩ gɩrɛ dɩɩ mɩɛ nɩ dɩ ga-n hɩɩna'.
60004013	Sɩ nɩ ka na kãkanɛ mɔ̃ nɩ bulni kha na gaarɛɛkɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ gaarnɩ, gɩ do nɔɔ dakha na-n kãka na daʋ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ wirəəkɛ na phananɩ.
60004014	A Kirisitii i do kɩrʋ dɩ wa nɩɩr nɩ ga-n da nar, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa Thuukɛ n nɛnanɩ mɔ̃ ɔɔ i dʋbɩ hanɩ ha narɛ.
60004015	Tibil nɛrɛra na-n gaar tɩɩ kʋdaar dʋʋrra ga, dɩ yudaar dʋʋrra ga, dɩ puu cʋʋdaar dʋʋrra ga, dɩ gɩrɛraakɛ na hɩɩrɛɛnaa ga,
60004016	sɩ ado Kirisitiida dʋʋrra gι, yicuru na-n fʋ nta', sι a ka na khιa Thãgba ireraalera.
60004017	Gιdonι bɔɔkɛ Thãgba na kɔɔ fʋnanι ɔɔ too kιιlɛ gι daan; dι ado sɛr ga kɔɔ fʋna ɓo, wιrɛ na-n nιɛnι Thãgbaa tutugo bʋɔɔ thιmιι nũə', mɔ̃ awιda na ha?
60004018	Gιdonι gι kherere Thãgbaa sɛbɛra ayι: “A gι sι fιιʋ sιι do tιι sarʋ na 'lɛ taara', dι mɔ̃ ga ha ʋrɛraakɛ na-n therananι Thãgba ga a dona sopugodaar?”
60004019	Gɛr gι wιrɛ n gaarɛnι mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba tuur hanι na-n jalana awι bɔ cʋʋra a gbana awι ha na pɛ thɩ̃ Tidaar bʋɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
60005001	Mι sor wιrɛraakɛ dɔnɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ anɩ pa, mɔ̃kɛ mɩ donɩ dakha kɔ̃tɩn awɩ kha, a tor yire Kirisitii bɔ gaarra, a dona dakha ʋrɛ na buloni kha na i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ na yɩranɩ,
60005002	nɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ kɔ̃tɩna mɩ so gɩrɛ ayɩ: Na-n khɛ Thãgbaa banaakɛ a pɛ narnɩ; na-n cʋʋ gɩ ho fɛrɛ pɛr ga, sɩ na-n cʋɛ na haar fɛʋ Thãgbara. Na-n khe wɩ warra ga, sɩ na-n khɛ wɩ na bɩ̃ bʋɔ.
60005003	Na-n cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ na fãga wɩrɛraakɛ wɩ pɛ narnɩ na-n hɩna', sɩ nɩ dɔ thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ banaana.
60005004	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ bana khedaar kɔ̃tɩn na ɩnɩ na 'lɛr khor cacadaar dʋʋrra, kɛ dɔnɩ i dʋbɩrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ dakʋɛnaa ga.
60005005	Mɛ̃ gɩ dakha na nɛr daɓola, nɩ jɔ dɩbara kɔ̃tɩnana. Nɛrɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl anɩ cʋʋ para nɩ hanana kha dɩbara jor, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa sɛbɛ sor ayɩ: “Thãgba n bãbaranɛ i ƴaaldara, sɩ a-n jɩrɛ dɩbara jodara bʋɔra.”
60005006	Gɛr gɩ na-n jɔ dɩbara Thãgbaa fãga nyɔ̃kɔɔ dɩ ɔr, a bɔɔ dã, a na ɩɩr nɛr.
60005007	Nɩ gba anɩ dɛsɔ fɛʋ a na faaraa gɩdonɩ ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ n hɩnɛ nɩnɩ.
60005008	Na-n jʋrɛ a na jɩɛ dʋ bʋrɛ, anɩ lãlaardaar Satã a-n kpaarɛ a ho sidũ'ũukɛ n huoneni, da-n ƴaalna ʋrɛ a na khonɩ.
60005009	Nɩ pɩɛrɛɛ kĩkĩ mɔ̃ nɩ jɩɩlnɩ kɩbɩ ha pɛrɛra, dɩ na-n jɛna gɩ dɩ bɔ gaar ca bɩɛlla anɩ omisɔ thɩɩraakɛ n yɩ.
60005010	Thãgbaakɛ bɔ jɩɩr fɛʋ n thernɩ, kɛ kɔɔ wɛ nɩnɩ nɩ bulo kha na ɔɔ khorr i dʋbɩ, gɩ the anɩ bɩɛl dora na Kirisiti, ado nɩ pɩ bʋɔɔkɛ nɩ-n gaarnɩ gɩrɛ bɔɔ gbe, a na cʋʋ nɛr dɩ na bɔr na ka, a na tɩ, a na hana dakha fãga, na ha tutugo paara'.
60005011	Ɔr hɩna fãga bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
60005012	Sɩlvɛ̃ɛkɛ mɩ-n wenɩ sobɔ omine, ɔr bulo mi dɩ ɩ̃ khere sɛbɛ buukɛ gɩ cʋʋ nι nι faa haar, ɩ̃ mιι nɩ dakha nɩ jɩɩ jɩ tue dɩ Thãgbaa bɔ jɩɩkɛra nɩ harɔnɩ bɔ jɩɩr gι gel, nι tɔɔ gar kɩbɩ.
60005013	We gbɛbιdaraakɛ hanι Babιlɔn, kɛ Thãgba phiirni anι kha, wι fʋɔr nɛr. Ɩ̃ bikuun Markɩ dakha fʋɔr nɛr.
60005014	Na-n fʋɔrɛ khasɔ na ha lõ fʋɔrɛ. Thãgba na-n hana nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ Kirisitira ha ɩɩ.
61001001	Mɛr Sɩmɔ̃ Pɩɛrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃daar na thɔ̃thɔn, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha nɛrɛɛkɛra 'lɛnɩ ha pɛ ca bɩɛlɩkɛ ɓɔnanɩ mɔ̃kɛ sɩ 'lɛ gɩnɩ, dɩɩ the Jeju Kirisitii fɩl sarra, kɛ dɔnɩ asɩ Thãgba a dona Taadaar.
61001002	Thãgba na-n jɛ nɩ bʋɔra jɔɔ, a na-n hana nɩ dakha ha ɩɩ jɔɔ, mɔ̃ nɩ-n jɩnɩ ɔr Thãgba na Jeju asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ dɩ ga-n pɛr.
61001003	Fãgaakɛ thɛnɩ ɔɔ Thãgba dora, gɛr hana sɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na bulo sini asɩ yi hanana na Thãgba fɩl hananɛna, gɩ the asɩ jɩraakɛ sɩ jɩnɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ wɛ sɩnɩ sɩ bulo kha na ɔɔ i dʋbɩ na ɔɔ bɔɔkɛ a bɔrnɩ,
61001004	kɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ nɔɔ dɩ ʋlfɛna sɩ ʋlfɛrɛsɔɔkɛ kɔ̃tɩnanɩ ka a ɓɔ̃ dakha ka, dɩ gɛrra na dɔ hʋɛ na yɩrɔnɩ a na debiro na do wɩrɛ na ɓananɩ kha na Thãgba ɔɔ Thãgba dora, mɔ̃ nɩ fuuni kʋɛrɛraakɛ ha pɩɛrɛ cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ lõ thɩɩraakɛ.
61001005	Dɩ gɛrra dɔ nɔɔ na-n gbɛ̃gbɛrɛnɛ dɩphã a hanana fɩl telẽe a dɛba anɩ ha pɛra, a hanana jɩɩr a dɛba fɩl teleena,
61001006	a hanana dɩbara fʋrɛ a dɛba jɩɩrra, a hanana yɩrrɛ a dɛba dɩbara fʋrɛra, a hanana Thãgba fɩlɛ a dɛba yɩrrɛra,
61001007	a hanana omi naar a dɛba Thãgba fɩlɛla, a hanana naʋ hulõo a dɛba omi naarra.
61001008	Gɩdonɩ ado ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ har anɩ bɩnɔ jɔɔ na too mɔlɔa', sɩ na-n cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ, na khʋɔn dakha na-n pɛr jɩɩrraakɛ nɩ jɩnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti.
61001009	Sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔka', yaarʋ a do, aa-n yɩ ƴɔa', a diinəne mɔ̃ Thãgba cɔcɔgɔɔnɩ ɔɔ sopugo tɩ̃sɔ.
61001010	Gɛr dɔ nɔɔ ɩ̃ omisɔ, na-n bãbanɛ a cʋɛ werɩkɛ Thãgba we nɩnɩ na phiireekɛ a phiir nini gɩ jɩɩ do thɩ̃ɛ phubi. Ado na cʋʋ mɛ̃ na tharsɩ na ji kpɩɩraka'.
61001011	Ga dor mɛ̃ Thãgba na ha nɩ hʋɛ kpẽgelẽ dɩ na lõ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na Taadaar Jeju Kirisitii khorr fãgadaar dɩra.
61001012	Gɛrra dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ɩ̃ ƴaal ma-n khe nar wire fɛʋ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ sɩɩ dorakɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lire jɩ gar a jɩɩl kɩbɩ sobɔrraakɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ.
61001013	Bɔɔraakɛ mɩ hanɩ gɩrɛ ɩ̃ waraakɛ, mɩ yɩɛrɛ dɩɩ bɔr dɩ ma khe nar ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛra gɩ jaa nar,
61001014	mɔ̃ mɩ jɩnɩ tue gɩrɛ dɩɩ ha mɔ̃kɛra asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ nɩ marnɩ, dɩ bɔɔkɛ ma thenɩ ɩ̃ warara ga hʋnɔa'.
61001015	Ma dor bʋɔ sɩ ɩ̃ cʋʋ thɩ̃ɛ, a mɩ kɔ̃ pɩ sɩ dɩɩ ha mɔnakɛ, sɩ na-n jɩna gɩ.
61001016	Ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ nɩnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii fãgada na ɔɔ bir ɩ̃ thɩmɩɩ, ga do kpuro nɩɛ 'lã'lã'lã sɩ kɔɔ pɛ nũu a gba a dιιrna na', sι wιrɛ kɔɔ yɛnι ɔɔ wabι na yire sι do.
61001017	Gιdonι a kɔɔ 'lɛr Thãgba Thιrɛra cʋrɛ na i dʋbιrɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ nʋɔ kɔɔ thenι carbara kʋkʋʋraale a so ayι: “Ʋrɛɛkɛra dʋɔn ɩ̃ Bikuunikɛ mι-n nanι, ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ lona mιnι haar ka.”
61001018	Sɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ kɔɔ nιɛnɛ na asι nũ nʋɔɔkɛ kɔɔ thɛnι ƴũ ɔbɔɔkɛ sι kɔɔ hanι kha na ɔr gɔ̃gɔ̃ phuurəəle.
61001019	Mɛ̃ sι jιɩ jι tue gel thιmιιrraakɛ Thãgbaa bobonasɔ kɔɔ mιɩnɩ; gɩ bɔrɛ dɩ na pɛ gɩ nũu, gɩdonɩ gɩ hʋrɛ lãphãakɛ n hɩrɛnɛnɩ pa birə paar phaphapha dɩɩ n wɩl, dɩwɩl ƴepələ̃bire n phã anɩ hara.
61001020	Sɩ caca thɩ̃ɛ, dɔ nɩ jɩ dɩ tibil na puno na ɔɔ thɛthɛɛ kpɩɛr na ti Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ kherenenɩɩ kɩra';
61001021	gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ kɔɔ thɛnɩ, ga do mɔ̃ tibili ƴaal hanɩ mɛ̃ gɩ kɔɔ ha kpɩɩraka', sɩ Thu Phuu kɔɔ cʋɛ tɩbɩla dɩ wɩ kɔɔ mɩɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa.
61002001	Mamara sõso bobona kɔɔ hale tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, mɛna gɩ sõso dɩɩrdara na wolone na lõ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn na sõso dɩɩrɛɛkɛ na bũburoneni tibil. Wa bor Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ kɔɔ thɛ wɩnɩ dɩ wa gbaar bũburoneekɛ na phuroneni tibil dapaara a na heen dɩbara.
61002002	Tibil jɔjʋɔ na kpar awɩ dakhaba thɔna, dɩ wɛr na dɔ nɔɔ dɩ tɩbɩla na mɩɩ dapuu wa-n pɛ sobɔ hʋɛra.
61002003	Ha pɩɛrɛ na cʋʋ wɛr dι wa gba sõso thιmɩɩr wɩ fɩɩlna nɩ wa-n 'lɛrɔ khor; sɩ gɩ maanɛ awɩ so heen hanɩ gbɛbɩrɔ, dɩ awɩ bũburõ ga do gɩ phɩnɛ daara'.
61002004	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba na kɔɔ sɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔraakɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ sopugoə', sɩ a kɔɔ fʋlɛ wɛr, a li a faa kõkor huloona dabirə paar tĩtĩtĩ gɩ dana kɩɩl wire.
61002005	Aa kɔɔ sɩrɔ dakha mama thɩa', sɩ a kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ yɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dɩɩ phã a thii tɩbɩla fɛʋʋkɛ na-n theranaana'; Noe dɩbara, kɛ n kɔɔ mɩanɩ tɩbɩla fɩl sar thɩmɩɩr, a kɔɔ taa na wɩ̃ tibil makonyɔ.
61002006	Dɩ dakha a kɔɔ heene Sɔdɔm na Gɔmɔɔrdara bũburõ so heene a thii wi na dɔɔ, a gba gɩ gɩrɛ da-n dɩɩrna wɩrɛ na-n theranaana' gɩrɛ na dana wɩnɩ.
61002007	A kɔɔ taarɛ dakha Lɔtɩ tɩɩ sarʋʋkɛ haar n helnɩ tɩɩ khabaasɔɔ cʋʋ pa kpalaale;
61002008	kũu sarʋʋlera kɔɔ hanɩ awɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, wire fɛʋ haar n heluu gɩdonɩ tɩɩ sarʋ a do, sɩ da-n yɩ awɩ cʋʋ pa puu da-n nɩɛna ga thɩmɩɩ dakha.
61002009	Wɩrɛ n cʋɔnnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn a-n jɩ gɛr da-n taa wɩ bɔ gaarɛra, sɩ dɩ thɩɩn wɩrɛ na sarana', a heen wɩ sor kɩɩl wirera.
61002010	Wɩrɛ n bɔnɩ dɩ wa-n ɩɩrna thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛkɛ n kɔnɩ awɩ tibil do pa thue, dɩ wa-n beesina dakha fãgaakɛ pɩɛrnɩ, wɛr ga bo na ɩɩrɔ. Sõso dɩɩrdaraale wɩ-n 'lar ka, wɩ gbɩllɛ, maar na-n kʋ wɩ ƴũ fãgadarasɔɔ kpɛra ga;
61002011	sɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛrakɛ hananɩ fãga na punone a jɔ wɩ, na tu na pɛ ƴũ fãgadarasɔɔle sor na kpɛɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩ ƴɛra ga.
61002012	Sɩ tibil ca wele wɩ hʋrɛ lɩɔ̃ nʋnɩaakɛ na hananɩ yʋa', kɛ wɩ kɔnɩ wɩ fɔ a na kɔ; wɩ-n kpɛr gɩrɛɛkɛ wa jɩna', nʋ̃ khaara wa bũburõ.
61002013	Wa 'lɛr bɔ gaarɛ gɩdonɩ mɛ̃ wɩ-n gaar tɩbɩla. Gɩrɛ n daan warnɩ dʋɔn wɩ tɔɔ gbelẽ gbelẽ a na cʋɛ puureekɛ n kɔ wɩnɩ thue. Jɩɩn tɩbɩla wɛ a khã; mɔ̃ wɩ-n hanɩ anɩ fɛtɩ cʋʋ pa dι wa-n fιιl nι gι-n da warɛ ka.
61002014	Khɛ kpιι ƴaal ƴιɛ wι hana; wa-n hi sopugo cʋʋra'; wι-n fιɩlɛ dakha tɩbɩlaakɛ na tɩɛnna'; ha pɩɛrɛ hi wer bɩnɔ; tɩbɩlaakɛ hanɩ sʋɔnna wɩ do.
61002015	Mɔ̃ wɩ faanɩ hʋ telẽe pɩ, wɩ buure dɩ wa-n kpaan Balam Bewɔɔrɩ bikuuni hʋra, kɛ kɔɔ naannɩ gõgolõ lɩmɩnɛ.
61002016	Sɩ a kɔɔ caananɛ phaanɛ ɔɔ puu cʋʋrara. Kũkə̃əkɛ na-n mιanι nʋɔa', sι a kɔɔ mιιraarɛ thιmιιr tibil khaa dιι cʋʋ bobon də̃bəl dι jιιl.
61002017	Tιbιlaale hor yɔ bu kanaakɛ na-n hananι nyʋɔna'; wι hor dakha thãgbaakɛ n jonanι sι dι jιɛ n ti gi; pa hulõ paarιkɛ birəneni tĩtĩtĩ Thãgba thιιn khorr dι ga-n pιɛr wι.
61002018	I ƴaal thιmιa na nɔfaar n thɛ wι nɔɔ. Thɩ̃ puukɛ n kɔnι tibil thue, kɛ dɔnι dakhaba thɔma wι gba dι wa-n fιιlna tιbɩlaakɛ fuonni fuu phaa a the sa faa wɩrɛ hanɩ sõsorra.
61002019	Dɩ wɩ-n so warɛ dɩ wɩ yɩ, ɩna cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wa do waɩa, sɩɩ do wɛr thɛthɛ dea wɩ do thɩɛnaakɛ na kʋɛa wɩnɩ, gɩdonɩ tibil n dor dee thɩɛnaakɛ jʋɔraanɩ.
61002020	Ado tɩbɩla fuu thɩɩkɛɛdaraakɛ n biseneni tibil pɩ, mɔ̃ wɩ jɩnɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na Taadaar Jeju Kirisiti, sɩ ado wɩ bir lõ ga thɩnaale dɩɩ puno wi, awɩ pɩpɩɩ pa na puurore a na jɔ cacadaa.
61002021	Mɔ̃kɛ wɩ jɩnɩ jɔfʋ phuukɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ha wɩnɩ sa gba faa, gɩ ka baarrakɛ ado wa ka kɔɔ jɩ fɩl sar hʋɛa'.
61002022	Gɩ dã warɛ waa mɔ̃kɛ sobɔ sokpaara hanɩ ger kɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ: “Bɩɩn n fire dɩ kho gɩrɛ a kɔɔ kpeenɩ”, dakha wo: “Sɩthookɛ wɩ-n cɔcɔɔnɩ n bire dapaara dɩ bɩɩr pɔɔsɔ.”
61003001	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, ʋrɛ dʋɔn balanyɔ sɛbɛɛkɛ mɩ khere narnɩ gɩrɛ. Sɛbɛ yenyɔraakɛ fɛʋ mɩ khe narɛ gɩ cʋʋ kpɩɛrɛ gɩ jaa nar;
61003002	dɩ mɛ̃ na jɩna gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa bobon phuusɔ kɔɔ maanɩ mɩɩrɛ, na Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ Taadaarɩ jɔfʋʋkɛ anɩ thɔ̃thɔna kɔɔ 'laanɩ.
61003003	Cacaca nɩ jɛna dɩ pɩpɩɩ wiresɔra ɓoɓorodara na ɩɩrɛ na maanɛ jɔɔ. Wɛr dɔ wɩrɛ n ɩrɛnɩ mɔ̃kɛ awɩ thɩ̃ puu ƴaal n kʋ wɩnɩ thue.
61003004	Wa sor nayɩ: Ɩɩnkɛra a kɔɔ yɩnɩ ɩna bire na ɩ̃, kana gɩ ha? Gɩdonɩ a fʋna wireekɛ asɩ thɩthɩsɔ kɔɔ khiirni, oti thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ too mɔnanakɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ti gini.
61003005	Sɩɩ do wɩ-n jɩrɛ gbobi, sɩ dɩ wɩ diinə, dɩ mamara nʋɔ Thãgba kɔɔ sona dɩ ƴũ na thɩɩkɛ hale gɩrɛ. Nyʋɔn a kɔɔ gba a cʋʋna thɩɩ dɩ nyʋɔnnana thɩɩ kɔɔ the.
61003006	Dɩ nyʋɔnna kɔɔ the thɩɩraakɛ kɔɔ hanɩle mamara dɩɩ kʋɛ.
61003007	Sɩ ƴũ na thɩɩkɛ hanɩkɛ nɛnɛ̃, thɩmɩɩ nɔ ca bɩɛlɩlera thɩnɛ gɩ, dɔɔ n kʋɛa gɩ wireekɛ dɔnɩ kɩɩl wire, kɛ wɩrɛ na-n therananɩ Thãgba ga na bũburoni.
61003008	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, thɩ̃ bɩɛl hale na-n diinə ga, gɛr dʋɔn, Kɔ̃tɩnna wi bɩɛl hor yɛna gbɩlanɩ, dɩ yɛna gbɩlanɩ ho wi bɩɛl.
61003009	Kɔ̃tɩn na-n pʋɔr sɩ dɩ cʋʋ gɩrɛɛkɛ a-n yɩnɩ ɩna cʋʋra', mɔ̃kɛ ɩkhasɔ n kpɩɛrnɩ gɩra', sɩ haar a-n fʋ nɛrɛra aa-n ƴaal tibil bɩɛl n buə', sɩ a-n ƴaalɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ n deba haar.
61003010	Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wi na daan mɔ̃ yu n ɩnɩ, ga Wiile thãgbara ƴũ na phor na ka na helle, dɩ ƴepələ̃be na mar dɔɔ a na hɩ̃ fɛʋ, dɩ thɩɩ na thɔmaakɛ n dʋɔnnɩ kɛ na thiire fɛʋ.
61003011	Dɩ gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛɛle fɛʋ thale ga kʋɛ, ʋmɔ̃ɔ tibil ca teana nɩ dɔ? Gɩ teenanɛ nɩ hanana fɩl phuu na Thãgba maar.
61003012	Na-n pɩɛrɛ sɩ nɩ phana dakha Thãgbaa wi gɩ dã, kɛ thãgbara ƴũ na donɩ dɔ haar a na hɩ̃ fɛʋ, ƴepələ̃be dakha n ma dɔɔ ga-n hɩl.
61003013	Ƴũ phaa na thɩ phaakɛ fɩl sarʋ na harɔnɩ sɩ-n pɩɛr, mɔ̃kɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ʋlfɛna sɩnɩ ɩna ha sɛr.
61003014	Gɛr gɩ, nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, mɔ̃ nɩ hanɩ pɩɛrɔ gɩrɛ, na-n bãbanɛ na-n do a yɩ nɩ na jiine na dɩ paara', sɩ nɩ dɔ a yɩ nɩ na ha ɩɩ.
61003015	Na-n jɛna dɩ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ha fʋ dʋɔn anɩ taa, mɔ̃kɛ Pol asɩ omiikɛ sɩ-n nanɩ kɔɔ khere narnɩ na kpɛsɛrɛɛkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ haanɩ.
61003016	Mɛ̃ a-n so ɔɔ sɛbɛsɔra fɛʋ ka a-n mɩɩnɩ ga thɩmɩɩ. Paar hale a khɩɩr jɩɩrra, dɩ jɩ 'leedara na wɩrɛ na tɩɛnna' n fi gi mɔ̃kɛ wɩ-n cʋʋnι na gɩ̃ Thãgbaa sɛbɛsɔ dakha, sι dιι do awι thɛthɛɛ kʋɛ gι.
61003017	Gɛr gι nɛrkɛ mι-n nanι, ne wer 'lire jιιr ga thɩ̃sɔɔle; na-n jιɛ hιιn dι tιι khabaasɔɔ fιl puu na-n cʋʋ nι nι lɛ̃ hʋɛra sι nι faa anɩ kɩbɩ jɩɩla'.
61003018	Nɩ jɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitiikɛ kɔɔ taa sɩnɩ ga-n pɛr, dɩ dɔ nɩ jɩ dakha bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ a kɔɔ jɩ sɩnɩ ga-n pɛr. Ɔr hɩna i dʋbɩrɛ nɛnɛ̃ waa, gɩ jalna khorr.
62001001	Gιrɛ kɔɔ hanι kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar, gιrɛ sɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ, gɩrɛ sɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ na asɩ yi dɩ sa-n hɩɩn, dɩ asɩ nyɛ̃ dakha kɔɔ tharrɔ, kɛ dɔnɩ yi thɩmɩɩ, gɛr sɩ khere nar.
62001002	Dɩ yireele kɔɔ yɩrrɛ dι sɩ kɔɔ yɩ gɩ, dɩ sa-n mɩɩ sobɔ so jɩɩr, dɩ yire khorrɩdara sɩ-n mɩɩ nɩ, kɛ kɔɔ hanɩ Thɩrɛɛ pa sa yɩr sar gɩrɛ.
62001003	Gelela sɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ a nɩɛna gɛr sɩ-n mɩɩ nɩ, dɩ mɛ̃ nɛrɛ dakha na do kha kũu bɩnɔ na sɛrɛ; dɩ ado sɛr gɩ sɩ dor kha kũu bɩnɔ na Thɩrɛ nakha ɔɔ Bikuun Jeju Kirisiti.
62001004	Dɩ sɩ-n kherere ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ dɩ mɛ̃ asɩ da na jɩɩ do daʋ na ka.
62001005	Dɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛra sι kɔɔ nιnι ɔɔ pa, dι sa-n mιι nι gιrɛ, gɛr dʋɔn Thãgba dʋɔn dahιrɛ, dabirə na haaraa fιιʋraka'.
62001006	Dι a sι so ayι, sι dor kha kũu bιnɔ na ɔr, sιι do dabirə sι-n jalna, sõsor sι kur, sa-n cʋʋ gιrɛ dɔnι sobɔra'.
62001007	Sι ado sι-n jaal na dahιrɛ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ hanι dahιrɛra, ga dor sι kuune khasɔ bιɛlbιɛl dι ɔɔ Bikuun Jejuu tɔmɩ̃ na-n cɔcɔɔ sɛr sopugo ɓibi.
62001008	Ado sι so ayι, sa hana sopugoə', ga dor dɩbara sɩ-n fɩɩl dɩ sobɔr na ha sara'.
62001009	Sɩ ado sɩ cã asɩ sopugosɔ, sobɔdaar Thãgba do, na fɩl sardaar, a na faa asɩ sopugosɔ na ha sɩ, sɩ a cɔcɔɔ sɩ asɩ thɩ̃ gõgolõ fɛʋ.
62001010	Dɩ ado sɩ so ayɩ, sa kɔɔ cʋʋ sopugoə', ga dor sõsodaar sɩ cʋgʋʋ dɩ do, dɩ ga dor ɔɔ so na haan asɩ bɩnɔa'.
62002001	Ɩ̃ bɩsã bi mɩ-n khere narɛ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ dɩ na-n cʋʋ sopugoə', sɩ ado tibil cʋʋ sopugo, sι hananɛ so ƴɛɛdaar Thιrɛɛ pa, Jeju Kirisiti fιl sardaar gι.
62002002	Dι ɔɔ thɛthɛra dʋɔn bonι jirikɛ hɛlanι asι sopugosɔ, ga do asι sopugosɔ dιbara ga, sι tɩbɩla fɛʋ thιιraada dakha.
62002003	Ado sι-n hιιnɛ ɔɔ jɔfʋ, liir sa jιι jɩna dɩ sɩ jɩɩrɛ.
62002004	Tibilikɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ, ɩnɩ jɩɩrɛ sɩ aa-n hɩɩn ɔɔ jɔfʋa', sõsodaar gɩ, dɩ dakha sobɔr na haaraa ga.
62002005	Ado tibil na hɩɩn ɔɔ so, ga dor Thãgba naʋ daan waa vʋ̃ʋ ntɛɛ pa, gɛr na cʋɛ sɩ dɩ sa jɩ tue dɩ sɩ haaraarɛ.
62002006	Dɩ tibilikɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ, ɔrra ɩnɩ too, gɩ teenanɛ ntɛ na-n ɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ kɔɔ ɩɩrnɩ.
62002007	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, ga do jɔfʋ phaa mɩ-n khere nara', sɩ jɔfʋ tɩ̃ɩ gɩɩkɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar, dɩ jɔfʋ tɩ̃ɩkɛra dʋɔn thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ.
62002008	Sɩrakɛ jɔfʋ phaa gɩ dɩ ɩ̃ khere nar, dɩ sobɔr gɩ do ɔrra na nɛrɛra, gɩdonɩ dabirə n kar sɩ dɩ dahɩrɛ bɔ 'li yɩrrɛ.
62002009	Tibilikɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ, ɩnɩ har dahɩrɛra, sɩ da-n laar ɔɔ omi, dabirəra a ha 'lo.
62002010	Tibilikɛ n naannɩ ɔɔ omi dahɩrɛra a too, dɩ nɛ baradaa na haaraa ga.
62002011	Sɩ tibilikɛ n laarɛnɩ ɔɔ omi dabirəra a ha, dɩ dabirərara a-n ɩɩr, dɩ aa jɩ kãkɛ a-n jalna', gɩdonɩ dabirə tɔnaa yɩr.
62002012	Mɩ khere narɛ bɩsã bii, gɩdonɩ ɔɔ i dɔ nɔɔ dɩ nɩ 'lɛ sopugo faarɛ.
62002013	Mɩ khere narɛ thɛ, gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ ʋrɛ kɔɔ hanɩle kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar. Mɩ khere narɛ daɓola, gɩdonɩ nɩ punone puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daar. Mι kɔɔ khere narɛ bιsana, gιdonι nι jιrɛ Thɩrɛ.
62002014	Mɩ kɔɔ khere narɛ thɛ, gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩrɛ ʋrɛ kɔɔ hanɩle kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar. Mɩ kɔɔ khere narɛ daɓola, gɩdonɩ nɩ hananɛ fãga, dɩ dakha Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ too nɛrɛra, dɩ nɩ puno puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daar.
62002015	Na-n do thɩɩkɛ na ɔɔda n bo ga-n too nɩ haara ga. A tibil na na thɩɩkɛɛ thɩ̃ aa-n hana naʋ Thɩrɛra ga.
62002016	Gɩdonɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hanι thιιra, kɛ dʋɔnnι thɩ̃ puukɛ n kɔnɩ tibil thue, na gɩrɛ n kɔnɩ yinə thue, na i ƴaalɛ thɩ̃ hananɛna, ga do Thɩrɛɛ pa gɩ tha', sɩ thɩɩra gɩ the.
62002017	Dɩ thɩɩra n kar na gɩrɛra n kɔnɩ tibil thue kɛ n thɩɛraanɩ, sɩ tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ Thãgba tuur n toore khorr.
62002018	Bɩsana, pɩpɩɩ bɔɔ ha gɩrɛ, dɩ mɔ̃ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ Kirisitii vardaar n ɩnɛ, nɛnɛnakɛ Kirisitii vardarasɔra jɔɔ hale, gɛrra sɩ jɩ dɩ pɩpɩɩ bɔɔ gɩ.
62002019	Wɩ kɔɔ ther asɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn, dɩ asɩda wɩ kɔɔ doraka'; gɩdonɩ ado asɩda wɩ kɔɔ do ga dor wa kɔɔ toona sɛr. Sɩ gele daan dɩ mɛ̃ ga nɩna dɩ bɩɛl na kɔɔ do asɩda ga.
62002020	Sɩ nɛrɛ, ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ Daphuu, Thu Phuu a kɔɔ ha nɩ, dɩ nɛrɛ fɛʋ jɩɩr na 'lee na'.
62002021	Mɩ kɔɔ khere narɛ gɩdonɩ ga do na jɩ sobɔraa ga, sɩ gɩdonɩ nɩ jɩ gɛr, dɩ sõso bɩɛllakɛ na the sobɔrra ga.
62002022	Amɛ dʋɔn sõsodaar saagado ʋrɛ n bananɛnɩ dɩ yɩ Kirisiti Jeju doaa ga; dɩ olela dʋɔn Kirisitii vardaar, ɔr n bɔ Thɩrɛ na Bikuun.
62002023	Tibil wo tibilikɛ n bɔnɩ Bikuun aa hana dakha Thɩra', sɩ tibilikɛ n tuonni Bikuun a hananɛ dakha Thɩrɛ.
62002024	Ado ne wer gɩ, nɩ dɔ gɩrɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar n too nɛrɛra; ado gɩrɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar n toore nɛrɛra, ga dor nɛrɛ dakha na toore Bikuunna na Thɩrɛra.
62002025	Dɩ ʋlfɛrɛɛkɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ kɔɔ ʋlfɛna sɩnɩ gɛr dʋɔn yire khorr.
62002026	Wɩrɛ n cʋɛ nɩnɩ dɩ na-n lɛ̃ hʋɛra dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ ɩ̃ khere nar ga thɩ̃ɩkɛ.
62002027	Ado nɛr gɩ, Thu Phuukɛ nɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ ɔɔ pa toore nɛrɛra, dɩ na hana ƴaalɛ ʋkha na-n dɩrɛ nɩ thɩ̃a', sɩ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ Thu Phuu n dɩɩr nɩnɩ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, na mɔ̃ a donɩ sobɔ sodaar ga do sõsodaar ga, nɩ tɔɔ ɔrra mɔ̃kɛra a kɔɔ dɩɩr nɩnɩ.
62002028	Dι nɛnɛ̃ bɩsã bii, nι tɔɔ ɔrra dɩ mɛ̃ wireekɛ a na phanɩ sa hananɛ 'lar, gɩ do ɔɔ bir ɩ̃ bɔɔ yicuru na fʋ sɩ sɩ hʋnɔnaa ga.
62002029	Ado nɩ jɩrɛ dɩɩ do fɩl sardaar a do, nɩ jɛ dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ dasarʋ ɔr kɔna ntɛ.
62003001	Nɩ yɛ naʋ caakɛ Thɩrɛ kɔɔ na sɩnɩ ɓoɓo dɩ wɩ thʋ̃ dɩ wa-n we sɩ Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔ, dɩ gɛrra sɩ do. Dɩ gɛrra dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ thɩdara na jɩ sa', gɩdonɩ wa kɔɔ jɩɩ dakha ga.
62003002	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔ sɩ do gɩrɛ, sɩ gɩrɛ sa donɩ ga yɩr pa'; sɩ sɩ jɩrɛ wireekɛ a na phanɩ sa hʋʋrɛ, gιdonι sa yιιrɛ mɔ̃kɛ a hanι.
62003003	Dι tibil wo tibilikɛ hananι nũ pɛ caakɛ n cʋʋrɛ dιbara a na-n phu mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ phuni.
62003004	Tibil wo tibilikɛ n cʋɛnι sopugo Thãgbaa jɔfʋ a-n kʋɛ, dι sopugo cʋʋrɛ dʋɔn jɔfʋ kʋɛrɛ.
62003005	Sι nι jιrɛ dι Jeju kɔɔ ιnɛ kɛ a ti asι sopugosɔ, dι ɔɔ thɛthɛra sopugo na haaraa ga.
62003006	Dι tibil wo tibilikɛ tɔɔnι ɔrra aa-n cʋʋ sopugoə'; tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ sopugo ntɛɛle na kɔɔ yɩa', aa kɔɔ jɩɩ dakha ga.
62003007	Bɩsã bii, na-n do tibil n fɩɩl na'; tibilikɛ n cʋɛnɩ dasarʋ, fɩl sardaar a do mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ thɛthɛ donɩ fɩl sardaar.
62003008	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛnɩ sopugo Satãa pa a the, gɩdonɩ Satã kɔɔ mãa fʋrɛ sopugo cʋʋrɛ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar, dɩ gɛr gɩ dɩ Thãgbaa Bikuun kɔɔ ɩ̃ a bũburõ Satãa thɔna.
62003009	Tibil wo tibilikɛ Thãgba kɔnɩ aa-n cʋʋ sopugoə', gɩdonɩ beekɛ Thãgba diirni har ɔɔ bɩnɔ, dɩ aa-n puno dɩ cʋʋ sopugoə', gιdonι Thãgba kɔnaa.
62003010	Gɩrɛ wɩ-n jɩnanɩ Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔ na Satãa bɩsãsɔ ha gɩrɛ: Tibil wo tibilikɛ na-n cʋɛnɩ dasarʋa', ga do Thãgbaada a doa', mɛna gɩ na ʋrɛ na-n naannɩ ɔɔ oma'.
62003011	Thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar gɛr ha gɩrɛ: Sa-n na kha fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
62003012	Dɩ sa-n ho Kayɛ̃ɛkɛ kɔɔ dɔnɩ puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩda, kɛ kɔɔ kɔnɩ ɔɔ õkuuna'. Dɩ mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ kʋʋ? Gɩdonɩ ɔɔ thɔ̃ puurore sɩ ɔɔ õkuunida sar.
62003013	Omɩna ado tɩbɩla thɩɩra na laar nɩ, na-n do nʋɔ n kpaa na'.
62003014	Sɛrɛ sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sɩ ther khirrə a lõ yirera, gɩdonɩ sɩ-n nar omɩna; ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ naʋa', khirrə a bo too.
62003015	Tibil wo tibilikɛ n laarɛnɩ ɔɔ omi tɩɩ kʋ haa, dɩ nɩ jɩrɛ dɩ tɩɩ kʋ bɩɛllakɛ na-n hana yire khorra'.
62003016	Sι jιrɛ gιrɛ n dɔnι naʋ, dι gɩ ther gιrɛraakɛ Kirisiti kɔɔ faa sarnι ɔɔ yi, sɛrɛ dakha gι teenanɛ sa-n faa asɩ yi omɩnana.
62003017	Ado tibil hana thɩɩkɛɛ thɩ̃ sa yɩ ɔɔ omi thɩ̃ ɓɔrɛra sɩ aa ƴaal a kher a hɩɩnʋa', mɔ̃ dɔ Thãgba naʋ haaraarɛ?
62003018	Bɩsã bii, sa-n na kha na nʋɔ dɩbara dɩ delẽbire ga, sɩ sa-n na kha na thɩ̃ cʋʋrɛ nakha sobɔr.
62003019	Gɛr sa jɩna dɩ sɩ dor sobɔdara, dɩ sa faarɛ haar yala ɔɔ ƴɛra.
62003020	Gɩdonɩ ado asɩ ha na heen sɩ sor, Thãgba kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ asɩ ha, dɩ a jɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ.
62003021	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, ado asɩ ha na-n heen sɩ sora', sɩ hananɛ tu jɩɩr Thãgbaa pa,
62003022	dɩ thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ sɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ a-n ha sɛr, gɩdonɩ sɩ-n hɩɩnɛ ɔɔ jɔfʋ dɩ sa-n cʋʋna gɩrɛ n daaraanɩ.
62003023	Dɩ gɩrɛ dɔ ɔɔ jɔfʋ ayɩ: Dɔ sɩ pɛr ɔɔ Bikuun Jeju Kirisitii i haar dɩ sa-n na kha fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl mɔ̃kɛ jɔfʋʋkɛ a kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ n sonɩ.
62003024	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n hɩnɛnɩ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ ɔr n tɔɔraa dɩ Thãgba n haaraa; dɩ Thu Phuukɛ a kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ sɩ jɩna dɩ a-n hana sɛr.
62004001	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, na-n pɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋʋda haara', sɩ na-n jʋrɛ wɩ na hɩnɛ ado Thãgbaa Thu n thɔɔ wɩ, gɩdonɩ sõso bobona jɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a lõ thɩɩra.
62004002	Gɩrɛ na jɩrɔnɩ dɩ Thãgbaa Thu gɩ: Tibil wo tibilikɛ n tuonni dɩ tomɩr Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ hana a ɩnɩ, Thãgbaa Thu ntɛɛle hana.
62004003	Sɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ na-n tuonni Jeju thala', ga do Thãgbaa Thu ntɛɛle hana ga, gɛr dʋɔn Kirisitii vardaarɩdara nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ ga ɩ̃, kɛ 'lenɩ hakɛrakɛ gɩrɛ thɩɩra.
62004004	Bɩsã bii, nɛrɛ, Thãgbaada nɩ do, dɩ nɩ puno wer, gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ hanɩ anɩ bɩnɔ a kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ hanɩ thɩdarara.
62004005	Wɛr, thɩɩda wɩ do, gɛr gɩ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ gɩrɛ thɩdara n mɩɩnɩ, dɩ thɩdara n pɛ wɛr nũu.
62004006	Sɩ sɛrɛ, Thãgbaada sɩ do. Ʋrɛɛkɛ jɩɛnnɩ jɩ Thãgba a-n pɛ sɛr nũu, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na dɔnɩ Thãgbaada ga, aa-n pɛ sɩ nũə'; liir sɩ-n jɩna sobɔ thue na fɩfɩɩl thue.
62004007	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, sa-n na kha fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl, gɩdonɩ naʋ Thãgbara gɩ the, dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ hananɩ naʋ, Thãgba kɔnaa dɩ jɩ Thãgba.
62004008	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ naʋa', aa jɩ Thãgba ga, gɩdonɩ Thãgba dʋɔn naʋ.
62004009	Gɩrɛ n nɛnanɩ naʋʋkɛ Thãgba na sɩnɩ dʋɔn mɔ̃ a kɔɔ thɔnɩ ɔɔ Bikũu bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ thɩɩra, dɩ mɛ̃ sa 'lɩɛraa yire.
62004010	Dɩ hɩnɛ mɔ̃ naʋra hanɩ, gɛr dʋɔn ga do sɛr kɔɔ naan Thãgba ga, sɩ ɔr gɩɩkɛ kɔɔ naan sɩnɩ a thɔ̃ ɔɔ Bikuun dɩ do sar bonɩ jirikɛ hɛlanɩ asɩ sopugo.
62004011	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, ado Thãgba kɔɔ na sɛr thale, gɩ teenanɛ sɛrɛ dakha sa-n na kha fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
62004012	Tibil na kɔɔ yɩ Thãgba yuuraka', sɩ ado sɩ-n nar kha fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl Thãgba har asɩ bɩnɔ, dɩ ɔɔ naʋ daan waa vʋ̃ʋ sɛrɛra.
62004013	Gɩrɛ sɩ jɩnanɩ dɩ sɩ tooraarɛ dɩ ɔr ha sɛrɛra dʋɔn gɩ ther gɩrɛraakɛ a kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ ɔɔ Thu.
62004014	Dɩ sɛrɛ, sɩ yɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ Thɩrɛ kɔɔ thɔnɩ ɔɔ Bikuun dɩ do tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩraa Taadaar, dɩ gɛr sɩ-n mɩɩrɔ sobɔ so jɩɩr.
62004015	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na tuonni nayɩ Jeju dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun, Thãgba haaraarɛ, dɩ ɔr dakha too Thãgbara.
62004016	Dɩ sɛrɛ, sɩ jɩrɛ naʋʋkɛ Thãgba hana sarnɩ dɩ sɩ pɛ gɛr haar. Thãgba dʋɔn naʋ, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnɩ naʋra a toore Thãgbara, dɩ Thãgba haaraa.
62004017	Mɔ̃ a hanɩ mɛ̃ sɩ ha ser thɩɩraakɛ, gelela dɔ nɔɔ dɩ naʋ dã waa vʋ̃ʋ asɩ bɩnɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ sa hana tu jɩɩr kɩɩl wire.
62004018	Naʋ na-n hana maara', sɩ naʋʋkɛ dananɩ vʋ̃ʋ n weere maar, gɩdonɩ maar n nɩnanɛ dɩ so 'lɛr n kpaanɛ, dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ maar n kʋnɩ na hana naʋʋkɛ dananɩ bɔɔbɔa'.
62004019	Ado sɛr gɩ, sɩ-n naarɛ gɩdonɩ ɔr kɔɔ naan sɩ caca.
62004020	Ado tibil so ayɩ, ɩnɩ-n nar Thãgba, sɩ na laar ɔɔ omi, sõsodaar gɩ; gɩdonɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n naannɩ ɔɔ omiikɛ a-n yɩna', mɔ̃ a na puno a na na Thãgbaakɛ aa yɩna?
62004021	Dɩ ɔrra sɩ 'lɛ jɔfʋʋkɛ ayɩ: Dɔ ʋrɛɛkɛ n naannɩ Thãgba a na-n na dakha ɔɔ omi.
62005001	Tibil wo tibilikɛ pɩɛrnɩ haar dɩ Jeju dʋɔn Kirisiti, Thãgba kɔnaa; dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ n naannɩ Thãgbaakɛ n kɔnanɩ tibil, a-n nar dakha ʋrɛɛkɛ Thãgbara kɔnɩ.
62005002	Sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sɩ-n nar Thãgbaa bɩsãsɔ ɔbɔɔkɛ sɩ-n nanɩ Thãgba dɩ sa-n cʋʋna ɔɔ jɔfʋ.
62005003	Gɩdonɩ Thãgba naar dʋɔn ɔɔ jɔfʋ hɩɩnɛ, dɩ ɔɔ jɔfʋra na khɩɩra'.
62005004	Gɩdonɩ ʋrɛ Thãgba kɔnɩ n punone thɩdaa; dɩ fãgaakɛ n punoneni thɩdaa dʋɔn asɩ ha pɛ.
62005005	Amɛ dɔ ʋrɛ n punoneni thɩdaa? Ʋrɛ dɩbara pɩɛrnɩ haar dɩ Jeju dʋɔn Thãgbaa Bikuun gɩ.
62005006	Ɔr dɔ Jeju Kirisitiikɛ kɔɔ ɩnanɩ na nyʋɔn na tɔmɩn, ga do nyʋɔn a ɩna dɩbara ga, sɩ nyʋɔn gɩ na tɔmɩn. Dɩ Thu Phuu dʋɔn ʋrɛɛkɛ n mɩanɩ sobɔ so jɩɩr, gɩdonɩ Thu Phuu dʋɔn sobɔr.
62005007	Gɩdonɩ yẽther hale n mɩanɩ sobɔ so jɩɩr:
62005008	Thu Phuu, nyʋɔn na tɔmɩn, dɩ wɛr yẽther dor kha nɔ bɩɛl.
62005009	Ado sa tu tɩbɩlaa sobɔ so jɩ, Thãgbaa sobɔ so jɩ kɔ̃tɩnɛ a jɔ gɩ, dɩ sobɔ so jɩɩrɩlera Thãgbaa thɛthɛ mɩa a pɛ ɔɔ Bikuunna.
62005010	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ haar Thãgbaa Bikuunna, a hananɛ ga sobɔ so jɩɩle ɔɔ bɩnɔ; sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na-n pɩɛrnɩ Thãgba haara', n cʋʋrɛ dɩɩ do sõsodaar Thãgba do, gɩdonɩ aa pɛr haar sobɔ so jɩɩrraakɛ Thãgba mɩɩnɩ a pɛr ɔɔ Bikuunna ga.
62005011	Dɩ hɩnɛ gɩrɛ dɔnɩ ga sobɔ so jɩɩkɛra, gɛr dʋɔn yire khorrɩkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ ha sɩnɩ, dɩ yireelera ɔɔ Bikuunna gɩ ha.
62005012	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ Bikuun a hananɛ yire, sɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ na hananɩ Thãgbaa Bikuuna', aa hana yirə'.
62005013	Mɩ khere narɛ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛ dɩ mɛ̃ na jɩɩ jɩ dɩ nɩ hananɛ yire khorr, nɛrɛɛkɛ n pɩɛrnɩ Thãgbaa Bikuuni i haar.
62005014	Tu jɩɩrɩkɛ sɩ hananɩ ɔrra dʋɔn, ado sa bɩɛlaa thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ do ɔɔ tuur gɩ, a-n pɛ sɛr nũu.
62005015	Dɩ ado sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ a-n pɛ sɛr nũu thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩɛnaakɛ sɩ-n bɩɛlnɩ, sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ sɩ 'lɛr thɩ̃ dookɛra sɩ kɔɔ bɩɛlaanɩ.
62005016	Ado tibil yɩ ɔɔ omi dɩ cʋʋ sopugookɛ na halaanɩ na jalna khirrə ga, a bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba omi dɔɔle na 'lɛr yire. A thɩɛna gaa, wɩrɛɛkɛ na-n cʋɛnɩ sopugookɛ n halanɩ dɩɩ jalna khirrə ga mɩ so. Sopugo hale n halanɩ tibil dɩɩ jalna khirrə, ga do ga sopugoole mɩ yɩ nɩ bɩɛllɔ Thãgba ga.
62005017	Thɩ̃ɛ wo thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na sarana', sopugo gɩ, sɩ sopugo hale na-n halanɩ tibil dɩɩ jalna khirrə ga.
62005018	Sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ tibil wo tibilikɛ Thãgba kɔnɩ aa-n cʋʋ sopugoə', gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa Bikuun n bɛraa, dɩ puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daar na-n thaaraa ga.
62005019	Sɩ jɩrɛ dɩ Thãgbaada sɩ do, sɩ thɩɩ koo puu cʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ gɩ ha.
62005020	Sɩ jɩrɛ dakha dɩ Thãgbaa Bikuun kɔɔ ɩnɛ kɛ a ha sɩ jɩɩr dɩ sa jɩna sobɔdaar; dɩ mɔ̃ sɩ hanɩ ɔɔ Bikuun Jeju Kirisitira, sobɔdaarra sɩ ha; ɔr gɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ sobɔ Thãgba a dona yire khorr.
62005021	Bɩsã bii, na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn, na-n ha kha dɩkha na thɩla fɩɩʋraka'.
63001001	Mɛr kɔ̃tɩn thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Kɩrɩa, kɛ dʋɔnnɩ khɛrɩkɛ Thãgba phiirni, a hana dakha ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ, kɛ dɔnɩ nɛrkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ na sobɔr, sɩ ga do mɛr dɩbara n naan na', sɩ wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ jɛnɩ sobɔr n naan nɩ,
63001002	dɩɩ the sobɔrraakɛ tɔɔnɩ sɛrɛra, kɛ na hanɩ kha na sɛrɛ na dana bɔɔ khorr.
63001003	Thãgba Thɩrɛ na Jeju Kirisitiikɛ dɔnɩ Thɩrɛɛ Bikuun na-n jɛ sɩ bʋɔra, a na-n dɔna sɩ dakha bʋɔ, a na-n hana sɩ dakha ha ɩɩ mɔ̃ sɩ donɩ wɩrɛ jɛnɩ sobɔr kɛ n naannɩ khasɔ.
63001004	Gɩ da marɛ haar ka dɩ ɩ̃ kɔɔ yɩ mɔ̃ afɩ bɩsã ɩkha n ɩɩrnɩ sobɔrra, mɔ̃kɛ jɔfʋʋkɛ sɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ Thɩrɛɛ pa hanɩ.
63001005	Dɩ nɛnɛ̃kɛ gɩrɛ mɩ-n ƴaal farnɩ Kɩrɩa, ga do jɔfʋ phaa mɩ-n khere fara', Sɩ gɩrɛra sɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar gɩ, gɛr dʋɔn sa-n na kha fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
63001006	Dɩ naʋ dʋɔn wɔɔ, sa-n ɩrɛ mɔ̃kɛ ɔɔ jɔfʋ hanɩ; gɛr dʋɔn jɔfʋʋkɛ teananɩ na-n ɩrɛrɔ mɔ̃kɛra nɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ kɛkɛkɛ fʋ paar.
63001007	Gɩdonɩ fɩfɩla jɔɔjɔɔ ɩɩrɛ a lõ thɩɩra, dɩ wa-n tu wɩ yɛ tomɩr Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ hana a ɩna'. Ʋrɛ hanɩ thale ɔr dʋɔn fɩfɩl na Kirisitii vardaar.
63001008	Na-n jɩɛ hɩɩn dɩbara dɩ gɩrɛ na 'lɛnɩ anɩ thɔna na-n do dakʋɛsʋa', sɩ nɩ 'lɛrɔ khor waɩ.
63001009	Ʋrɛ n ɩrɛnɩ da-n kəəro si aa-n too Kirisitii dɩɩrra ga, aa hana Thãgba ga. Sɩ ʋrɛ tɔɔnɩ dɩɩrɛraakɛ, ɔr hana Thɩrɛ na Bikuun.
63001010	Ado tibil pɔ anɩ pa, sɩ ga do dɩɩr ca ʋrɛ a pɔna ga, na-n teguu a to cʋɔrɔa', na-n fʋɔrʋʋrakɛ dakha ga.
63001011	Gɩdonɩ ntɛɛkɛ na fʋɔrɛɛnɩ ɔɔ thɔ̃ puusɔ a tu.
63001012	Mɩ hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ a na khere nar gbobi, sɩ ma ƴaal ɩ̃ gba sɛbɛ na sɛbɛ khere nyʋɔn ɩ̃ mɩɩna na', sɩ mɩ-n pɛrɛ haar ɩ̃ pɔ anɩ pa sɩ mɩɩ kha ƴɛ biro, dɩ mɛ̃ asɩ da na jɩɩ do daʋ na ka.
63001013	Afɩ õkhɛrɩkɛ Thãgba phiirni, ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ fʋɔr fɛr.
64001001	Mɛr kɔ̃tɩn thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha Gayʋsɩɩkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ. Mɩ-n naarɛ na sobɔr.
64001002	Ɩ̃ kuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, mɔ̃ mɩ-n ƴaalnɩ gɩ hana far dʋɔn, thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ na-n jala far bɔɔ, fɩ 'lɛ tomɩ kheu, mɔ̃ afɩ thuda n jalnɩ bɔɔ.
64001003	Gɩ da marɛ haar ka, ɔbɔɔkɛ omɩna kɔɔ ɩnɩ a mɩɩ sobɔ so jɩɩr sobɔrraakɛ hanɩ afɩ pa, kɛ dɔnɩ mɔ̃ fɩ-n ɩɩrnɩ sobɔrra.
64001004	Ma hana daʋ dɩɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ jɔ da ʋra', kɛ dɔnɩ mɔ̃ mɩ-n nɩɛnɩ dɩ ɩ̃ bɩsãsɔ n ɩɩrɛ sobɔrra.
64001005	Ɩ̃ kuunikɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, fɩ-n cʋʋrɛ bɔɔ gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ-n cʋʋnɩ omɩnana, narakɛ omɩnanaakɛ dɔnɩ kpakpala.
64001006	Wɩ mɩɩrɛ sobɔ so jɩɩr afɩ naʋra we gbɛbɩdaraa thɩ̃thɩɩn; ga bɔrɛ ado fɩ bul wi na fɩlɛɛkɛ na danɩ Thãgbara awɩ kpaar para.
64001007	Gɩdonɩ Jeju Kirisitii i dɔ nɔɔ wɩ thenι jal, sɩ wa-n tee thɩ̃ɛ ca kpalaa pa ga.
64001008	Gɛr gɩ sɛrɛ, sɩ teenanɛ sɩ tea wa tibil casɔɔle, a gbɛba kha thɔma na dɔ sobɔrra.
64001009	Mι kɔɔ kherere thɩmιιr gbe a ha we gbɛbιdara, sι Diyotιrɛfιιkɛ n ƴaalɛnι ιnι-n dɔ war ƴɛ kʋl aa-n gba asιda ga.
64001010	Gɛr gι ado mι pɔ, cʋʋ caalera a-n cʋʋnιsɔ ma ιιrna gɛr, gιdonι a-n mιιrɛ thιmιι puunə da-n pɛ sar, sι gelelakɛ ga-n nιιraa pa', sι ɔɔ thɛthɛ n yι, ιna tee omιna ga, dι wιrɛ n ƴaalɛnι wa-n cʋʋ wo a-n pιɛr wɛr, sι dι wee wι we gbɛbιdaraa thɩ̃thιιn da-n faa.
64001011	Ɩ̃ kuunikɛ mι-n nanι, fa-n phɛl thɩ̃ puə', sι na phɛla thɩ̃ bʋɔ. Ʋrɛɛkɛ n cʋɛnι gιrɛɛkɛ bʋɔnɔnι Thãgbaada a do, sι ʋrɛ n cʋɛnι gιrɛ puurohi aa yι Thãgba ga.
64001012	Tιbιla fɛʋ na sobɔrι thɛthɛrakɛ n mιιrɛ so jι bʋɔ dι wa-n pɛ Demetiriynsira; sɛrɛ dakha sι-n mιιrɛ so jιιr dι sa-n pιɛraa, dι fι jιrɛ asι so jι dʋɔn sobɔr.
64001013	Mι hananɛ thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ a na khere far, sι ma-n ƴaal ɩ̃ gba sɛbɛ khere nyʋɔn na sɛbɛ kheredaa ɩ̃ mιιna fa'.
64001014	Sι mι pɛrɛ haar kιɛr na gbe ma yι fɛr sι mιι kha ƴɛ biro.
64001015	Thãgba na-n hana fι ha ιι. Asι kuunsɔ fʋɔr fɛr; fʋɔrɛ asι kuunsɔ fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl na awι i.
65001001	Mɛr Juudiikɛ dɔnɩ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃daar, a dona Jakɩɩ õkuun, thɔna sɛbɛɛkɛ a ha wɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgba Thɩrɛ wenɩ a na na wɩ dakha, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ Jeju Kirisiti n bɛrnɩ.
65001002	Thãgba na-n dɔna nɩ bʋɔ jɔɔ, a na-n hana nɩ dakha ha ɩɩ jɔɔ, a cʋɛ nɩ nɩ jɩɩ jɩ ɔɔ naʋ jɔɔ.
65001003	Nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, ƴaalɛɛkɛ mɩ kɔɔ hananɩ ɩ̃ hara dʋɔn ɩ̃ khere nar sɛbɛ taarɛraakɛ sɩ bulni khaa thɩmɩɩra, dɩ mɩ yɩ gɛr dɩɩ do dɔ ɩ̃ khere nar ger phubi ɩ̃ kpãkpãa nar nɩ kɛ̃kɛrɛ̃ na-n pɛ ha pɛdaaraakɛ tɩɩ phuusɔ 'lɛnɩ babɩɛl khorr.
65001004	Gɩdonɩ ɩkhaa tibilsɔ kɔɔ wolone a lõ anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn; tɩbɩla wɛɛkɛ na-n therananɩ Thãgba ga, wɩ debire Thãgbaa bɔ jɩ thɩmɩɩ ga-n jala mɔ̃kɛ awɩ khaakhaar thɩ̃ cʋʋ hanι, wι bor dakha Jeju Kirisiti asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ bιɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽekɛ dɔnι fãgadaar. Wɛr dɔ tιbιlaakɛ awι so heen kɔɔ maanι kherere.
65001005	Nɛrkɛ jιɛnnι ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera fɛʋ mɔ̃kɛ gι hanι, sι mι-n ƴaalɛ ɩ̃ bir ɩ̃ khe nar wo nι jιna dι ɔbɔɔkɛ Kɔ̃tιn kɔɔ taanι ɔɔ too Ejipiti dιιra pι, wιrɛ na kɔɔ pιɛnι haara', a kɔɔ bũburõ wer.
65001006	Nι jɛna dakha dι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛ kɔɔ faanι gιrɛ wι pɛ warnι, wa kɔɔ too dakha awι pa ga, a kɔɔ li wer khorr a faa dahulõ paar dabirəra, phaphapha gι dana wi kɔ̃tɩ̃ιkɛ a na kιιlna wιnι.
65001007	Nι jɛna dakha Sɔdɔm na Gɔmɔɔr na awι dι khudaraada, kɛ kɔɔ faanι awιbara bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra oti, dɩ wa-n cʋʋna gɩrɛ Thãgba na kɔɔ tini tibil a cʋɛa'; wɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr so heene khorr dɔɔra, dɩ gɩrɛra dana wɩnɩ dor gɩrɛ thɩ̃ nɩrɔrɛ tɩbɩlala fɛʋ.
65001008	Mɛna tɩbɩlaale n yɛnɩ thɩ̃ɛ ɩnɩ yɩ ha dakha, awɩ tomɩ wɩ-n bise, wɩ-n beesire dakha Kɔ̃tɩnɩ fãga hana dɩ wa-n kpɛna ƴũ fãgadarasɔ.
65001009	Mɩsɛlɩkɛrakɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, ɔbɔɔkɛ sʋʋ kɔɔ ιιrnι dι wa-n bana kha na Satã Mʋιjιι forra, sιrakɛ aa kɔɔ heenuu sor na kpɛra', sι gιrɛ a sʋʋraanι dιbara dʋɔn: Kɔ̃tιn n pɛ far sor.
65001010	Sι tιbιlaale wer, gιrɛ wa jιnιnaka' wι-n kpɛ gɛr, sι gιrɛ wι jιnι hɔ̃ nʋ̃ khaa dιι do mɛ̃ gι-n do, gɛr dɔ gιrɛ na kʋɛa wιnι.
65001011	Ga puu warɛ dɛ, gιdonι Kayɛ̃ɛ hʋ wι gba a lona dakha dι paarra war ƴaalɛla Balamι kha, wι bũburone mɔ̃ wι ιιrnanι lãʋ Koree kha.
65001012	Pheru wɩ do mɔ̃ wɩ-n hanɩ anɩ naʋ dɩko kho pa sɩ dɩ wɩ gɔ lõ khaakhaar cʋʋrɛra, sɩ yicuru na-n fʋ wa'; wa-n therna tibil saagado awɩbara gaaga. Wɩ hʋrɛ thãgbaakɛ n jonanɩ sɩ dɩ jɩɛ n ti gi; wɩ hʋrɛ dakha thɩraakɛ dananɩ sɩɩr sɩ ga-n sa'; thɩr khɩna yɛɛkɛ wɩ phiirni faa.
65001013	Wɩ hʋrɛ lanyʋɔnɩkɛ jɩɛ na-n sɩrɔnɩ cɔcɔa', awɩ yicur thɔ̃ cʋʋ n ther yɔkhɔrɔ̃ khaa. Wɩ hʋrɛ dakha ƴepələ̃beekɛ n fileneni bababa; pa hulõ paarιkɛ birəneni tĩtĩtĩ Thãgba thιιn khorr dι ga-n pιɛr wι.
65001014	Sι Enɔkι, mama kɔ̃tιn, kɛ dɔnι makonyɔdaarιkɛ Adã karɔnι sι dι kpaan, a kɔɔ mιιrɛ awιda dιι do bʋʋr gι dι bo ayι: “Kɔ̃tιn ιnɛ na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ tə̃tə̃tə̃,
65001015	a kιιlna tιbιla fɛʋ, a heen wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na-n theranaana' sor, gι the awι thɔ̃ puurəəkɛ wι kɔɔ cʋʋnι Thãgbara, na awι thιmιι kpallaakɛ wɛr sopugodaraalera na-n theranaana' kɔɔ mιιraanι.”
65001016	Tɩbɩla wɛɛkɛ hũhuune donɩ awɩda na cɩ̃cɩmanɛ; wɩ-n ɩɩrɛ mɔ̃ awɩ ha pɩɛr hanɩ; i ƴaal thɩmɩɩ haar n thɛ wɩ nɔɔ; wɩ-n fɩɩlɛ tɩbɩla wa-n 'lɛrɔ khor.
65001017	Sɩ nɛrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ omɩnaakɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, na-n jɛna thɩmɩaakɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii thɔ̃thɔ̃sɔ kɔɔ maanɩ mɩɩrɛ.
65001018	Wɩ-n kɔɔ so narɛ ayɩ: A pɩpɩɩ bɔɔ na dã, wɩrɛɛkɛ na-n maanɛ nɩnɩ na hale, wa-n ɩɩr mɔ̃kɛ awɩ thɩ̃ puu ƴaal n kʋ wɩnɩ thue.
65001019	Wɛr dɔ tɩbɩlaakɛ na-n pɩɛrnɩ leere; thɩɩkɛɛda wɩ do, wa hana Thãgbaa Thuə'.
65001020	Sɩ nɛrɛɛkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ, nɩ khɔna na pɩɛr anɩ ha pɛ bɔraakɛ nɩ hananɩ; na-n bɩɛlnɛ Thãgba na Thu Phuu fãga.
65001021	Nɩ jɩɛ too naʋraakɛ Thãgba na sɩnɩ, mɔ̃ nɩ-n pɩɛrnɩ yire khorrɩkɛ asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisiti na ha nɩnɩ, gɩ do ɔɔ bɔ donana gɩ the.
65001022	Wɩrɛ n ƴeƴerenenɩ na-n bulo wi;
65001023	na-n taa wɩ a vənə wi dɔɔra na te; ɩkhasɔ wo, na-n jɛ wɩ bʋɔra sɩ nɩ dɔ gɩ do bɔ jɩɩrɩkɛ hananɩ maar, nɩ thʋ̃ na-n laarnanakɛ khələlələ kɩ̃kɩɩnɩkɛ thɩ̃ puu ƴaalɛɛkɛ n kɔ wɩnɩ thue cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ bise.
65001024	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na punoneni na fʋ nɩ dɩ na jə', a cʋʋ nɩ dakha nɩ jɩɩlna kãkar ɔɔ ƴɛraakɛ n carbaranɛnɩ, nɩ 'lee dɩ paar;
65001025	ʋrɛɛkɛra dɔnɩ Thãgba bɩɛl dɩbara gɩ, kɛ kɔɔ taa sɩnɩ dɩɩ do asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ Jeju Kirisitii pa gɩ the, dɔ gɩ do ɔr hɩna i dʋbɩrɛ, na wabɩrɛ, na fãga, na punone, bɔɔ fɛʋraakɛ kɔɔ kanɩ, na nɛnɛ̃, na bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
66001001	Gɩrɛɛkɛ dʋɔn nɩrɔrɛɛkɛ Thãgba kɔɔ hanɩ Jeju Kirisiti a gba nɛna Thãgbaa thɔ̃darasɔ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na dananɩ kɔrɔ. Dɩ Kirisiti thʋɔn ɔɔ thɔ̃daar thu a cʋɛ ɔɔ thɔ̃daar Jã a jɩ gɩ,
66001002	kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ mɩanɩ gɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ a yɩnɩ, kɛ dɔnɩ thɩmɩɩrɩkɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa na sobɔrɩkɛ Jeju Kirisiti kɔɔ mɩgʋʋnɩ.
66001003	Ga dar ʋrɛraakɛ n hɩnɛnɩ sɛbɛɛkɛ na wɩrɛraakɛ n pɛnɩ Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ nũu, dɩ wa-n nɩ nũu dakha gɩrɛraakɛ kherenenɩ, gɩdonɩ bɔɔkɛ ga thɩ̃sɔɔkɛra na danɩ gɩ daan.
66001004	Jã thɔna fʋɔrɛɛkɛ a ha we gbɛbɩdaraa cɔ makonyɔɔkɛ hanɩ Ajɩ ayɩ: Bɔ jɩɩr na ha ɩɩ n dana nɩ, kɛ n thɛnɩ Thãgbaraakɛ hanɩle gɩrɛ, kɛ dakha kɔɔ hanɩle, kɛ na ɩnanɩ, kɛ n thɛnɩ dakha thue makonyɔraakɛ hanɩ ɔɔ fãga too pa ƴɛ bʋrɔ,
66001005	kɛ dakha n thɛnɩ Jeju Kirisitii pa, kɛ dɔnɩ sobɔ so jɩdaar, na cacadaarɩkɛ Thãgba kɔnɩ, kɛ kɔɔ ɩrɛnɩ a the khirera, kɛ dɔnɩ gɩrɛ Fãgadaar kpɩɛ fãgadarara kɛ thɩɩra. Ʋrɛɛkɛ naan sɩnɩ a thʋbɩ sɩ sopugo pɔ̃ɔ na ɔɔ tɔmɩ̃,
66001006	ɔr gɩɩkɛ kɔɔ cʋɛ sɩnɩ dɩ sɩ do fãgadaraakɛ dɔnɩ bonɩ jidara Thãgbaraakɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ Thɩ, dɔ ɔr n hɩ̃ i dʋbɩrɛ na fãga bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
66001007	Hɩnɛ a-n ɩnɛ na ndɔlɔ̃pana, dɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ na yɩɩrɛ narakɛ wɩrɛ kɔɔ gʋɔnɩ na khalʋ, dɩ tibil caar fɛʋ thɩɩra na-n bɩrɛ ɔɔdara. Sobɔr gɩ thalera ga ha. Amɛn.
66001008	Mɛr dʋɔn Alfa na Omega, Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar, kɛ hanɩle gɩrɛ, kɛ dakha kɔɔ hanɩle, kɛ na ɩnanɩ, mɛr sɔ.
66001009	Mɛr Jã anɩ omiikɛ buloni kha na nɛrɛ bɔ gaarɛ, na fãgadaar dɩɩ, nakha yɩrrɛ dɩɩ do asɩ bɩɛl dora na Jeju gɩ the, mɩ kɔɔ har yɔ dɩɩraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Patɩmɔsɩ gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa thɩmɩɩ na sobɔrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Jejuuda mɩ-n kɔɔ mɩɩ.
66001010	Thu Phuu kɔɔ ɩɩrna mɛr Kɔ̃tɩnɩ wi dɩ mɩ kɔɔ nɩrɛ nɔ khɩɩr ɩ̃ khiro dɩɩ ho mɔ̃ wɩ-n ʋnɩ tutuu,
66001011	dɩɩ so ayɩ: Gɩrɛra fɩ yɩnɩ, khera gɩ sɛbɛra, a thɔna hana we gbɛbɩdaraa cɔ makonyɔɔkɛ hanɩ Efɛjɩ, na Sɩmɩrnɩ, na Pɛrgam, na Tɩatɩɩr, na Saardɩ, na Fɩladɛlfɩ, na Laʋdɩse.
66001012	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ kɩɩlɛ ɩ̃ hɩɩn wi dɔɔlera n mɩana mɩnɩ, dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɩɩlnɩ, mɩ yɩrɛ dɔ carã dɛ̃ɛ paarɩkɛ dɔnɩ dɛdaa makonyɔ,
66001013	dɩ tibil hale a jɩɩl thɩ̃thɩɩn da-n hona tibili bikuun, a to kẽkẽ gbãa dɩɩ dã nɛɛ, sa khɩmɩ dɛ lo phɛrɛ kũkuno.
66001014	Ɔɔ yʋsũ bulolole phɩphɩphɩl a ho phũgə̃, a hona dakha mɩlɛ, sɩ ɔɔ yisɔ hʋrɛ dɔlɩnanɛ.
66001015	Ɔɔ nɛsɔ n carbararɛ mɔ̃kɛ the sɩɛ n hɩlnɩ dɔɔra, sɩ ɔɔ nɔ so pa ho yɔ jɔ helle.
66001016	Ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra ƴepələ̃be makonyɔ hale dɩ fʋrɔ, dɩ khalgbãakɛ n khɛnɩ bilə yenyɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ hale a thɩɩ nʋɔra, sɩ ɔɔ ƴɛ wer hʋrɛ mɔ̃ wire n carbaranɩ ʋlkhɔɔ.
66001017	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ yɩɩnɩ mɩ jire ɔɔ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn a ho khire, sɩ a tha marɛ na nyɔ̃bɔɔ sa so ayɩ: Fa-n do maar n fʋ fa'. Mɛr dɔ cacadaar na pɩpɩɩdaar,
66001018	a dona yidaar. Mɩ kɔɔ khire, sɩ hɩnɛ mɩ hananɛ yire gɩrɛ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ, dɩ mɛr n punone khir na khĩdi dɩɩ dakha.
66001019	Gɛr gɩ khera gɩrɛɛkɛra fɩ yɩnɩ, kɛ hanɩle gɩrɛ, na gɩrɛ na pɩrɔnɛnɩ na kpaan.
66001020	Ado ƴepələ̃be makonyɔɔdaakɛ fɩ yɩnɩ ɩ̃ nyɔ̃bɔra gɩ, na dɔ carã dɛ̃ɛ paarɩkɛ dɔnɩ dɛdaa makonyɔɔda, thɩ̃ gbul gɩ, dɩ ga kɩr dʋɔn: Ƴepələ̃be makonyɔɔle dʋɔn thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛ hanɩ we gbɛbɩdaraa cɔ makonyɔ, sɩ dɔ carã dɛ̃ɛ paar makonyɔɔle dʋɔn we gbɛbɩdaraa cɔ makonyɔ.
66002001	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Efɛjɩ we gbɛbɩdaraada. Hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ fɔrɔnɩ ƴepələ̃be makonyɔ ɔɔ nyɔ̃bɔra, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ n kpaarɛnɩ dɔ carã dɛ̃ɛ paarɩkɛ dɔnɩ dɛdaa makonyɔɔ thɩ̃thɩɩn sonɩ ayɩ:
66002002	Mɩ jɩrɛ afɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ, na afɩ thɔ̃, na afɩ ha fʋ. Mɩ jɩrɛ mɔ̃ fa-n punoni a na bɔ kha na puu cʋʋdara ga. Wɩrɛ yɛnɩ thɔ̃thɔna ɩnɩ do sɩɩ do wa doa', fɩ kɔɔ be wer bɩnɛ a hɩɩn a yɩɛ dɩɩ do sõsodara wɩ do.
66002003	Fɩ hananɛ ha fʋrɛ, fɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ dakha haar bʋɔraakɛ fɩ kɔɔ gaarnɩ dɩɩ do ɩ̃ i dɔ nɔɔ sɩ fa kɔɔ vɔa'.
66002004	Sɩ sorɩkɛ mɩ hana fɩnɩ dʋɔn mɔ̃ fɩ faanɩ naʋʋkɛ fɩ kɔɔ hananɩ cacara.
66002005	Jɛna ka fɩ thenɩ ɓoɓo a thʋ̃ ji sa deba haar, a birə na cʋɛ afɩ caca thɔ̃, agado mɛ̃ ga, ma pɔ farɛ dɩ ma gbaar afɩ dɔ carã dɛ̃ɛ pa, agado haar fɩ deba'.
66002006	Sɩ gɩrɛ fɩ hananɩ wer dʋɔn mɔ̃ fɩ-n laarnɩ Nɩkolayɩtɩsɔɔ thɔ̃ khələlələ, kɛ dɔnɩ thɔmaakɛ mɛrɛɛ thɛthɛ n laarnɩ dakha.
66002007	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra. Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni, ma haarɛ hʋɛ dɩ na kho yi thɩrʋʋ biikɛ hanɩ hɩɩr paar Thãgbaa kal ƴɔɔ.
66002008	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Sɩmɩrnɩ we gbɛbɩdaraada. Hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ cacadaar na pɩpɩɩdaar, kɛ kɔɔ khenɩ sa bir ɩɩr a hana yire sonɩ ayɩ:
66002009	Mɩ jɩrɛ afɩ bɔ gaar na afɩ bɔdaar do phuphuphul, sɩɩ dorakɛ lẽledaar fɩ do. Mɩ jɩrɛ dakha i kʋɛrɛɛkɛ wɛkɛ yɛnɩ Juifisɔ ɩnɩ do n kʋɛ fɩnɩ, sɩɩ do wa do Juifisɔa', Satã wɩ-n kpa jɛ a na fʋɔr.
66002010	Fa-n do maar n fʋ fɩ gɩrɛraakɛ fa gaarna'. Hɩnɛ Satã na cʋʋrɛ dι wa fʋlɛ ιkhasɔ anι thɩ̃thιιn a na to khaιra gι be nι bιnɛ gι hιιn, dι na gaarɛ bʋɔ wire yʋɔr. Dɔ sobɔ cʋʋdaar a danana khir dɩ fa 'lɛr ɩ̃ pa khorɩkɛ dɔnɩ yidaa.
66002011	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra. Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni, balanyɔ khir na puno na cʋgʋʋ thɩ̃a'.
66002012	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Pɛrgam we gbɛbɩdaraada. Hinɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ khalgbãakɛ n khɛnɩ bilə yenyɔ fɛʋ sonɩ ayɩ:
66002013	Mɩ jɩrɛ ka fɩ-n cɔnɩ, dɩ liir Satãa fãga too pa ha, sɩ fɩ fʋrɔrɛ ɩ̃ i. Ãtɩpasɩɩ bɔɔrakɛ, sɩ fa kɔɔ faa ha pɛrɛɛkɛ fɩ hana marna'. Ãtɩpasɩra sobɔ tibil a kɔɔ do mar da-n mɩɩ ɩ̃ dabɔ, dɩ wɩ kɔɔ kʋʋ anɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn kãkɛ Satã n cɔnɩ.
66002014	Sɩ dɩ pa ɩkhaakɛ mɩ yɩ farnɩ dʋɔn mɔ̃ ɩkhaa tibilsɔ hanɩ afɩ pa, dɩ wɩ bo dɩ wa-n ma Balamɩ dɩɩrra, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ kɔɔ dɩrɛnɩ Balakɩ dɩ pɛr bara paar Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsanana dɩ wa kho thɩl thɩ̃ɛ, a na faana dakha dɩbara bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra.
66002015	Mɛna gɩ ha gɩrɛ dakha, fɩ hananɛ tɩbɩla afɩ pa kɛ n bɔnɩ dɩ wa-n ma Nɩkolayɩtɩsɔɔ dɩɩrra.
66002016	Gɛr gɩ deba haar dɛ, ado mɛ̃ ga, ma pɔ farɛ kɔrɔ a na kɛ̃kɛrɛna wɩ na ɩ̃ nɔ khalgbã.
66002017	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra. Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni ma haarɛ maan kɛ keranɩ, ma haarɛ dakha boka bulo, dɩ boka bulolaalera i phaa na khere, kɛ tibil na jɩnɩ saagado ɔrkɛra 'lɛnɩ gaaga.
66002018	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Tɩatɩɩrdaraada. Hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thãgbaa Bikuunikɛ ɔɔ yisɔ honɩ dɔlɩnanɛ, dɩ nɛɛ na-n carbara mɔ̃kɛ the sɩɛ n hɩlnɩ dɔɔra sonɩ ayɩ:
66002019	Mɩ jɩrɛ afɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ, na afɩ naʋ, na afɩ ha pɛ, na afɩ thɔ̃ do, na afɩ ha fʋ, na afɩ nɛnɛ̃ thɔ̃ɔkɛ jɔnɩ mamadaa.
66002020	Sɩ sorɩkɛ mɩ hana fɩnɩ dʋɔn mɔ̃ fɩ sɩnɩ khɛrraakɛ wɩ-n wenɩ Jejabɛl, kɛ yɛnɩ khɛ bobon ha nɩ, da-n dɩɩr da-n fɩɩlna ɩ̃ thɔ̃daarsɔ dɩ wa faa dɩbara bɔdɛl cʋʋrɛra, wa-n kho dakha thɩl thɩ̃ɛ.
66002021	Mɩ kɔɔ haarɛ bɔɔ dɩ a na debi haar, sɩ aa-n ƴaal a deba haar ɔɔ bɔdɛl cʋʋrara ga.
66002022	Fa yɩ gaa, ma tʋɔrɛ na kpɛɛ phɩ̃ paar sɩ ɩ̃ thɔnanaa bɔ gaarɛ, gɩ wabɩ na wɛkɛrara n phɩnanaanɩ dakha. agado haar wɩ debi a faa ɔɔ thɔ̃ɔlera ga.
66002023	Ma cʋʋrɛ ɔɔ bɩsãsɔ dɩ wa khiir, dɩ we gbɛbɩdara fɛʋ na jɩrɛ dɩ mɛr dʋɔn bɩɛlɩkɛ n bəəreni tibili kpɩɛr na ɔɔ ha, dɩ ma 'laa narɛ fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl thɩ̃ɛ mɔ̃ anɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ hanɩ.
66002024	Sɩ ado nɛrkɛ sɛnɩ Tɩatɩɩr, kɛ na-n tuonni ga dɩɩrɩla', kɛ na jɛnɩ thɩ̃ dookɛ welela n wenɩ Satãa thɩ̃ hulõə', ma gba heenda kpɩɩ na heen nɩ bã;
66002025	sɩ gɩrɛ nɩ hananɩ, nɩ jɩɛ fʋ gɩ kĩkĩkĩ phaphapha ɩ̃ pɔ.
66002026	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ fɔrɔnɩ ɩ̃ thɔ̃ a dana khu paar, ma haarɛ punone tibil caarra,
66002027	dɩ ga ha mɔ̃kɛra mɩ 'lɛ gɩnɩ ɩ̃ Thɩɩ nyɔ̃kɔɔ, dɩ “ɔr na khɛ wɩ na the gbʋʋl, a na-n cɔ wɩ khʋma khʋma ce khaa”,
66002028	dɩ ma haarɛ dakha dɩwɩl ƴepələ̃bire.
66002029	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra.
66003001	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Saardɩ we gbɛbɩdaraada. Hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ hɩnanɩ Thãgbaa Thu makonyɔ na ƴepələ̃be makonyɔ sonɩ ayɩ: Mɩ jɩrɛ afɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ. A wɩ yɩ fɩ wɩ-n ka jɩna yidaar ha fɩ sɩɩ do fɩ khire.
66003002	Jaga a cʋɛ gɩrɛ sɛnɩ sɩ dɩ ga-n jal khiir paar gɩ hana yire, gɩdonɩ ma yɩ afɩ thɔ̃ dɩɩ thʋ̃ bɔr a dã thu ɩ̃ Thãgbaa ƴɛra ga.
66003003	Jɛna gɩrɛ fɩ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ a nɩɛna, dɩ na ɔ gar sa deba haar. A fa jaga, ma ɩnɛ yudaar khaa, dɩ fa jɩ bɔɔkɛ ma phuro fina'.
66003004	Sɩ ɩkhasɔ hale anɩ thɩ̃thɩɩn le Saardɩ, kɛ na kɔɔ biseneni awɩ kẽkẽsɔa'. Wɛr na-n ɩrɛ kha na mɛrɛ na kẽkẽ bulona gɩdonɩ wɩ teena gɛr.
66003005	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni a na 'lɛr kẽkẽ bulo a na to, dɩ ma pɩɩn ɔɔ i yi sɛbɛra ga, sɩ ma caan ɩ̃ Thɩɩ ƴɛra na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔ ƴɛra nayɩ ɩ̃da a do.
66003006	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra.
66003007	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Fɩladɛlfɩ we gbɛbɩdaraada. Hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ daphuu na sobɔdaar, ʋrɛɛkɛ fɔrɔnɩ Davɩdɩɩ lakile, ʋrɛɛkɛ n khɛranɩ dɩ tibil na-n puno dɩ khaana', kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ n khaanɛnɩ dɩ tibil na-n puno dɩ khɛra' sonɩ ayɩ:
66003008	Mɩ jɩrɛ afɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ. Afɩ fãga na kpɛra', sɩɩ do fɩ kɔɔ fʋrɛ ɩ̃ nɔ, fa kɔɔ bananɔ ɩ̃ iə'. Hɩnɛ mɩ faarɛ loo dɩɩ khɛr hoo afɩ ƴɛbʋrɔ, kɛ tibil na punoni na khaana'.
66003009	Hɩnɛ gɩrɛ ma cʋʋnɩ wɩrɛɛkɛ n kpanɩ jɛ a na fʋɔr Satã, kɛ n sõsonenɩ dɩ wɩ yɩ, Juifisɔ ha nɩ, sɩɩ do wa do Juifisɔa', ma cʋʋ wɛr dɩ wa tha na thʋnɔ sɩ na gburõku far, dι wa jιrɛ dakha mι na fɛr.
66003010	Gιdonι fι kɔɔ fʋrɛ ɩ̃ nɔ a hana ha fʋrɛ, mɛrɛ dakha ma bɛr fɛr bɔ gaar bɔɔkɛ na ιnanι na gba thιιkɛ koo gι be tιbιla bιnɛ gι hιιn.
66003011	Ma ιnɛ kɔrɔ. Jιɛ fʋ gιrɛ fι hananι kĩkĩkĩ, dι mɛ̃ tibil na taa far khorιkɛ fa 'lɛna'.
66003012	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni ma cʋgʋʋrɛ dɩ na do thɩkarʋ cʋɔrraakɛ dɔnɩ ɩ̃ Thãgbaada, dɩ a na the le bã. Ma gbaar ɩ̃ Thãgbaa i a na khereraa, na ɩ̃ Thãgbaa dɩɩ i, kɛ dɔnɩ Jerujalɛm phaakɛ thɛnɩ ɩ̃ Thãgbaa pa ƴũ a gbũ, ɩ̃ kherenanaa dakha ɩ̃ i pha.
66003013	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thu Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra.
66003014	Khera thakɛ a hana thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ Laʋdɩse we gbɛbɩdaraada. Hɩnɛ gɩrɛɛkɛ ʋrɛɛkɛ dɔnɩ Amɛn, a dona sobɔ so jɩdaar bʋɔ, a dona Thãgbaa thɩ̃ tinə fɛʋʋ the pa sonɩ ayɩ:
66003015	Mɩ jɩrɛ afɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ. Fa ɩa', fa kpora'; mɩ-n ƴaalɛ fɩ ie agɩbo fɩ kpor.
66003016	Sɩ gɩdonɩ fɩ har bɔnɔnɔnɔ, fa ɩa', fa kpora', ma kpee fer na faa.
66003017	Gɩdonɩ fɩ sor ayɩ, fɩ ler aa, thɩ̃ɛ fɩ 'lɛ a le, dɩ dakha wo thɩ̃ɛ na-n ɓɔr fa', sɩɩ do fa jɩ dɩ fɛrɛ, fa do tibiləə ga, bɔ kʋ tibil ha fɩ, fɩ dor dakha bɔdaar bulo, a dona yaarʋ, a hanana sãɓɔlɔ̃.
66003018	Gɛr gɩ mɩ-n ha fɛr fɩlɛ, a fɩ jɩ thɛ mar dɛɛkɛ wɩ thiini dɔɔ dɩɩ bɔr, mɛ̃ fa debi na do lẽledaar dɩphã; na kẽkẽ bulo dakha fɩ to fɩ kɛɛna yicuru, tibil na yɩ afɩ sãɓɔlɔ̃a'; na dakha wo yi thɩɩkɛ fa pɛnɩ yiro fɩ puno fa-n yɩ.
66003019	Mɛrɛ, wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ mɩ-n nanɩ wɛr mɩ-n nɩna dɩ paar dɩ ma-n wɛbɩna wɩ. Gɛr gɩ hanana ƴaalɛ jɔɔ a deba haar.
66003020	Hɩnɛ, mɩ hakɛ a jɩɩl lõfonɔɔ dɩ ma-n be. Ado tibil nɩ ɩ̃ nɔ, a khɛr mɩ loo, ma lʋʋn na too ntɛɛ pa sa-n kho kha dɩkɔ.
66003021	Ʋrɛɛkɛ na kəəneni ma haarɛ hʋɛ da too kha na mɛrɛ ɩ̃ fãga too para, mɔ̃kɛ mɛrɛ dakha kəəni sa too gɩrɛ na ɩ̃ Thɩ ɔɔ fãga too para.
66003022	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ nũu, dɔ a na-n nɩ gɩrɛɛkɛ Thʋ Phuu n sonɩ we gbɛbɩdarasɔra.
66004001	A gele pɩ, mɩ-n kɔɔ hɩɩnɛ dɩɩ do lõfonʋɔ gɩ a khɛr Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩ caca nʋɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ nɩɛnɩ dɩ a-n mɩɩna mɩ a ho tutuu ʋʋn gɩ so marɛ ayɩ: Jʋnɛ kɛ, ma nɩ farɛ gɩrɛ teananɩ gɩ dana bɔɔraakɛ na kpaanɛnɩ.
66004002	Dapaara Thu Phuu kɔɔ ɩɩrna mɛr dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ fãga too paar dɩɩ hale Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩ tibil hale a too fãga too paarraalera.
66004003	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛra kɔɔ tɔɔrɔnɩ n carbararɛ jasɩpɩ boka khaa na sardʋan boka khaa, kɛ dɔnɩ bokanaakɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ ka, dɩ thãgba khalʋ kɔɔ hale a dii fãga too paarraalera dɩ a-n hona emərodi bokaarɩkɛ khiinoni dakha the nʋɔ ka.
66004004	Dɩ fãga too pa kpelẽ yenã hale a dii fãga too paarraalera, dɩ kɔ̃tɩna kpelẽ yenã hale a too fãga too paarsɔrara, a to kẽkẽ bulona, a suunə dɛ fãgadaar kpɩɛr yʋɔ.
66004005	Dɩ thãgba jʋ khor, na nɔ khena, na thãgba tiire n ther le fãga too paarraalera; dɩ lãphã makonyɔ hale a do dɔ haar dɩ ga-n le fãga too pa ƴɩɛraalera, gɛr dʋɔn Thãgbaa Thu makonyɔ.
66004006	Dɩ fãga too pa ƴɩɛraalera thɩ̃ɛ hale dɩ ga-n hona lanyʋɔn wɩwɩwɩl sa ho hɩɩnʋ. Dɩ fãga too pa thɩ̃thɩɩn thɩ̃ ye yenã hale a diiro, dɩ yinə hire awɩ tomɩra ƴɛbʋrɔ na khiru fɛʋ.
66004007	Caca thɩ̃ yire hor sidũ'ũu, balanyɔ thɩ̃ yire ho na ɓolʋ, balãther thɩ̃ yire hana tibil ƴɩɛ, sɩ balanã thɩ̃ yire ho gbʋɔrɛɛkɛ n dɩɛnnɩ.
66004008	Dɩ thɩ̃ ye yenãale bɩɛlbɩɛl hananɛ gbɛla maadõ maadõ, wɩ hinəne yinə bɩnɔ na tomɩrra dakha, dɩ wa hana pɩrrɛ kpɩɩ dɩwɩlʋ na dɩtɩnɔa', sɩ mɛ̃ wɩ-n so aa: “Daphuu, daphuu, daphuu, Thãgba Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar do, kɛ kɔɔ hanɩle, kɛ hanɩle gɩrɛ, kɛ na ɩnanɩ.”
66004009	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ thɩ̃ yeele n dʋbɩnɩ ʋrɛ tɔɔnɩ fãga too paar, kɛ hɩnanɩ yire bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ, dɩ wa-n kpãganaa, dɩ wa-n khɩɩnaa,
66004010	kɔ̃tɩna kpelẽ yenãale gburõkure ʋrɛraakɛ tɔɔnɩ fãga too paarraale ƴɩɛra, dɩ wa-n fʋɔr ɔrkɛra hɩnanɩ yire bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ, dɩ wɩ phubire awɩ fãgadaar kpɛsɔ a kpɛɛ fãga too pa ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn sɩ wa-n so:
66004011	Asɩ Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na asɩ Thãgba wei, fɛr teana a na 'lɛ i dʋbɩrɛ, na cʋʋr, na punone; gɩdonɩ fɛr kɔɔ te thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ, dɩ afɩ tuur dɔ nɔɔ dɩ gɩ hale gɩrɛ a hana yire.
66005001	Dɩ mɩ yɩrɛ sɛbɛ dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnɩ fãga too paar thɛbɩ na nyɔ̃bɔɔ, dɩɩ khere bɩnɔ na jɩɛra fɛʋ, dɩ jena makonyɔ hale a dʋrɔ dɩɩ do gɛr khaanɛ gɩ.
66005002	Dɩ mɩ yɩrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ hananɩ fãga dɩɩ və̃vĩə, dɩ hulẽ nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka ayɩ: Amɛ teana a na cʋɔr jɩɩnsɔɔle dɩ sɛbɛɛle na phubi?
66005003	Dɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na hale Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩ thɩɩra gɩ, dɩ thɩɩraakɛ tɩɛr gɩ, a na puno na phubi sɛbɛra ga, a na puno dakha wo a na hɩɩna'.
66005004	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ khɩɩrɛ jɔɔ ka gɩrɛraakɛ tibil na yɩnɩ, kɛ teananɩ a na phubi sɛbɛra agɩbo a hɩɩna'.
66005005	Sɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl kɔ̃tɩnanaalera so marɛ ayɩ: Fa-n khɩa'. Hɩnɛ sidũ'ũukɛ thɛnɩ Judaa cara, a dona Davɩdɩɩ məl, ɔr kəəne a na cʋɔr jena makonyɔɔlera sɩ na phubi sɛbɛra.
66005006	Dɩ mɩ yɩrɛ fãga too pa thɩ̃thɩɩnɩle, na thɩ̃ ye yenãale, na kɔ̃tɩnaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, Bana bii dɩ jɩɩl le sa ho mɔ̃ wɩ kʋʋnɩ, sɩ a hananɛ ʋma makonyɔ na yinə makonyɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa Thu makonyɔ, kɛ a thɔnɩ thɩɩraakɛ koo.
66005007	Dɩ a pɔr, a tee sɛbɛɛle olelaalera hana gɩnɩ a fʋrɔ nyɔ̃bɔɔra a toona fãga too paarra.
66005008	Ɔbɔɔkɛ a teenɩ sɛbɛɛle pɩ, thɩ̃ ye yenãale, na kɔ̃tɩna kpelẽ yenãale gburõkure Bana bɩɩ ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn; wɛr fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl kɔɔ fʋrɔrɛ salãa na dɛ bilẽse dɩɩ hinə latɩkolookɛ dɔnɩ tɩɩ phuusɔɔ Thãgba bɩɛl.
66005009	Dɩ wɩ khɩnɛ nɩ phaakɛ sɔnɩ ayɩ: Fɛr teana fɩ tee sɛbɛra fɩ cʋɔr dakha jɩɩnsɔ, gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ kʋ fɛr dɩ fɩ gba afɩ tɔmɩ̃ a birsena tɩbɩla, caarra fɛʋ, na thɩmɩɩrra fɛʋ, na tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ thɩ̃thɩɩn, na ca kpalala fɛʋ a ha Thãgba.
66005010	Fɩ cʋʋ wɛr dι wι do fãgadaraakɛ dɔnι bonι jidara asι Thãgbara, dι wa dor fãgadara thιιra.
66005011	Dι mι-n kɔɔ hιιnɛ a nιɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu jɔjʋɔɔ wi, kɛ awι ther nɔ kanιkɛ gbιlanι der paar gbιlanι, wι thʋnɛ və̃vĩə, a dii fãga too paarra, na thɩ̃ yera na kɔ̃tιnanaale,
66005012	dι wι so na nɔ kheu ayι: Bana biikɛ wι kɔɔ kʋnι a teenanɛ a 'lɛ punone, na ler, na kpɛsɛrɛ, na fãga, na cʋʋr, na i dʋbιrɛ, na khιιrɛ.
66005013	Dɩ thɩ̃ tinəne fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, na thιιra, na thιιraakɛ tιɛr, na lanyʋɔnna, na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ harɔnι bιnɔ, mι nιɛrɛ dι wele fɛʋ na-n so ayι: Ʋrɛ tɔɔnι fãga too paar na Bana bii, dɔ ɔr n hɩ̃ khιιrɛ, na cʋʋr, na i dʋbιrɛ, na fãga bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ.
66005014	Dι thɩ̃ ye yenãale dee aa: Amɛn. Dι kɔ̃tιnaale gburõku dι wa-n fʋɔr.
66006001	Dι mι yιɛrɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ Bana bii kɔɔ cʋɔrnι caca jιιn jena makonyɔraale, mι nιɛrɛ thɩ̃ yi bιɛl thɩ̃ ye yenanaale dι so nʋɔ dιι ho thãgba phɛɛrɛ ayι: Ɩna.
66006002	Dι ma hιιn dιι do gãgo bulo gι a the, dι ʋrɛ kɔɔ jʋnɛɛnι kɔɔ hananɛ thaa na tʋʋ, dι wι haarɛ fãgadaar kpιɛr dι a ther mɔ̃ a donι kəkəədaar a 'lɛ kəəre.
66006003	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a cʋɔrnι balanyɔ jιιn, mι nιɛrɛ balanyɔ thɩ̃ yire dι so: Ɩna.
66006004	Dι gãgo sιɛ khəkhəkhə ther, dι ʋrɛ jʋnɛɛnι kɔɔ 'lɛr punone a na tinə ha ιι thιιra na faa, dι mɛ̃ tιbιla na-n kʋʋr kha; dι a 'lɛr dakha bajιna kɔ̃tɩ̃ι.
66006005	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ cʋɔrnι balãther jιιn, mι nιɛrɛ balãther thɩ̃ yire dι so ayι: Ɩna. Dι ma hιιn a yι gãgo biru, dι ʋrɛ jʋnɛɛnι fʋrɔrɛ thɩ̃ mιɛdaa ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
66006006	Dι mι nιrɛ nʋɔ dιι the thɩ̃ ye yenãa thɩ̃thιιnιle a so ayι: Jʋ mιɛ nɔ bιɛl, gɛr dɔ wi bιɛl thɔ̃ lιmιnɛ; ɔljʋ mιɛ nʋɔ yẽther, gɛr dɔ wi bιɛl thɔ̃ lιmιnɛ; sι niin wer na taan, fa-n cʋʋrɔ thɩ̃a'.
66006007	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ cʋɔrnι balanã jιιn, mι nιɛrɛ balanã thɩ̃ yire dι so ayι: Ɩna.
66006008	Dι ma hιιn a yι gãgʋʋkɛ hanι phʋaphʋa, dι ʋrɛ jʋnɛɛnιι i n dʋɔn khir, dι khĩdi dιι na-n kpaaraa sιkaar, dι wι 'lɛr punone a na gbana bajιna, na kɔmɛr, na kho puu, na hɔ̃ nʋma thιιra a na bũburona tιbιla thι phɛrɛ yenana bιɛlbιɛl.
66006009	Dι ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ cʋɔrnι balamɔι jιιn, mι yιrɛ tιbιlaa thusɔ bonι ji pa ballɔ, kɛ dɔnι wιrɛ wι kɔɔ kʋʋrnι Thãgbaa sora, na awι sobɔdaar doraakɛ wι jιιlnι.
66006010	Dι wι hulene dιι khιιr ka ayι: Kɔ̃tιn, daphuu na sobɔdaar, ka ga dã sι fa kιιl kιιlʋ a na tiir asι tɔmɩ̃ hel thιdarara?
66006011	Dι wɛr fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl 'lɛr kẽkẽ bulo gbana a to, sι dι wι so war ayι, wι tɔɔ ɓo cɔcɔcɔ phaphapha wιrɛ dɔnι thɔ̃ dona awι kha, na awι omisɔɔkɛ wa kʋʋrnι awι kha, awι nɔ n dã ɓo.
66006012	Dɩ mɩ yɩɛrɛ ɔbɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ cʋɔrnɩ maadõ jɩɩn, thɩ jɩɩn kɔɔ hale a kɔ̃tɩ̃ ka, dɩ wire debire a biiro tĩtĩtĩ a ho bʋ bir lokaar, dɩ por biləni debi a sɩɛrɔ a ho tɔmɩn.
66006013	Dɩ ƴepələ̃be na-n jɛ thɩɩra, mɔ̃kɛ jɩɛ na-n və̃viləni thɩr khonanɛ dɩ bi pholoo na-n jɛ.
66006014	Dɩ thãgbara ƴũ pur kʋla kʋla mɔ̃ wɩ-n purni dɛbɛ, dι gɔ̃gɔnasɔ fɛʋ na yɔ dιιsɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ əəle a ha dιkhãa pa.
66006015	Dι le fãgadara thιιra, na kɔ̃tιnasɔ, na sɔrasɛɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔ, na lẽledara, na fãga hɩ̃dara, na dea ɓibi, na waιasɔ n wɔ̃ wιwιl kanana na boka kɔ̃tɩ̃ ballɔsɔɔkɛ hanι gɔ̃gɔnana;
66006016	sι wa-n so gɔ̃gɔnana na boka kɔ̃tιnana ayι: Nι je the sarrakɛ a phe sι, sι hʋnɔna ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnι fãga too paar na Bana bii nĩkhirə.
66006017	Gιdonι awι nĩkhi wi kɔ̃tɩ̃ phaan, dι ʋmɔ̃ hale na jιιl?
66007001	A gele pι, mι yιrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu yenã dι wι jιιl thι khu paar yenã, sa fʋ jιɛ yenãakɛ n thɛnι thιιra a fʋrɔ, dι mɛ̃ jιɛ na-n the thιιra, dι lanyʋɔnna gι, dι thιr bιɛlla gιraka'.
66007002	Dι ɩ̃ bir yι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpιι wo dι the wi phã paar da-n jʋʋn, a fʋrɔ Thãgba yidaarι jẽ pɛda sa hulẽ nʋɔ dιι khιιr ka thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu yenanaale kɔɔ 'lɛnι hʋɛ a na cʋʋna thιι puure na lanyʋɔn,
66007003	a so ayι: Na-n cʋʋ thιιra puure na lanyʋɔn pa', dι thιra ga, phaphapha sι pɛ asι Thãgbaa thɔ̃darasɔra jιιn kobera ɓo.
66007004	Dι mɩ nɩrɛ wɩrɛ wɩ pɛrnɩ jɩɩnnaa nɔ dɩ wɩ yɩ tɩbɩla gbɩlanɩ tamaa na kpalanyɔ na gbɩlanɩ yenã wɛ, kɛ thɛnɩ Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsanaa cara fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl.
66007005	Judaa cara, gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ wɩ dʋrɔ jɩɩnna, Rubɛnɩ cara, gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ, Gaadɩɩ cara, gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ,
66007006	Ajɛɛrɩ cara, gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ, Nɛfɩtalɩɩ cara, gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ,
66007007	Manasee cara, gbɩlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ, Sɩmɛ̃ʋʋ cara, gbιlanι yʋɔr yenyɔ, Levιι cara, gbιlanι yʋɔr yenyɔ,
66007008	Ɩsakaarι cara, gbιlanι yʋɔr yenyɔ, Jabʋlɔ̃ɔ cara, gbιlanι yʋɔr yenyɔ, Jojɛfιι cara, gbιlanι yʋɔr yenyɔ, Bɛ̃jamɛ̃ɛ cara, gbιlanɩ yʋɔr yenyɔ, wɩ dʋrɔ jɩɩnna.
66007009	A gele pɩ mɩ-n kɔɔ hɩɩnɛ dɩɩ do tibil jɔ wɛ tə̃tə̃tə̃, kɛ tibil na punoni na thera', a the ca kpalala fɛʋ, na caarra fɛʋ, na tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ thɩ̃thιιn, na thɩmɩɩrra fɛʋ, dɩ wa-n jɩɩl fãga too pa ƴɩɛra na Bana bii ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, a to kẽkẽ bulo gbana sa fʋrɔ kalã jɛ̃ɛ nyɛɛna.
66007010	Dɩ wɩ-n hulene nɔ khena ayɩ: Asɩ Thãgbaakɛra tɔɔnɩ fãga too paar, ɔrra taarɛ n the na Bana biirə.
66007011	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ fɛʋ jɩɩlɛ a dii fãga too paarra, na kɔ̃tɩnana, na thɩ̃ ye yenana, a gburõku fãga too pa ƴɩɛra dɩ wa-n fʋɔr Thãgba,
66007012	dɩ wa-n sona ayɩ: Amɛn. Khɩɩrɛ, na i dʋbɩrɛ, na kpɛsɛrɛ, na fʋɔrɛ, na cʋʋr, na punone, na fãga, asɩ Thãgba hɩna bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Amɛn.
66007013	Dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ bɩɛl kɔ̃tɩnanaale bule mi ayɩ: Welela tɔnɩ kẽkẽ bulo gbana, ana wɛ dɩ ka wɩ the?
66007014	Dɩ ɩ̃ sʋʋraa: Ɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ya mee fɛr ka jɩ gɩ. Dɩ a so marɛ ayɩ: Wɛr dʋɔn tɩbɩlaakɛ thɛnɩ bɔ gaar kɔ̃tɩɩnaale; wɩ kɔɔ cɔcɔɔrɛ awɩ kẽkẽsɔ a cʋʋ gɩ na Bana bii tɔmɩ̃ dɩɩ bulolo.
66007015	Gɛr dɔ kɩrʋ dɩ wɩ ha Thãgbaa fãga too pa ƴɩɛra, dɩ wa-n dʋʋraa thɔma dɩwɩlʋ na dɩtɩnɛ ɔɔ cɔra; dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnɩ fãga too paarra na dʋrɛ ɔɔ wa na thi war.
66007016	Kɔmɛr na fʋ wɩ bã, yɔlkhaa na fʋ wɩ bã, dɩ ɩtʋɛ na dakporuu na 'lɛ wɩ dakha bã.
66007017	Gɩdonɩ Bana biikɛ hanɩ fãga too pa thɩ̃thɩɩn na-n khɛ wɩ a thɔɔ wɩ a na-n jalna yi yɔ bu kanana, dɩ Thãgba na pɩɩnɛ yilẽbe fɛʋ awɩ yirə.
66008001	Ɔbɔɔkɛ Bana biirə kɔɔ cʋɔrnɩ makonyɔ jɩɩn, pɩrrɛ kɔɔ hale Thãgbaa dʋɔ a cʋ lɩɛr kuru.
66008002	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ Thãgbaa thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔɔkɛ n jɩlɛnɩ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, dɩ wɩ 'lɛr tutuu makonyɔ.
66008003	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ pɔr a jɩɩl bonɩ ji pa kɩrɔ, a hana latɩkolo 'wiidaakɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ dɛ; dɩ a 'lɛr latɩkolo jɔɔ a gba a na-n 'laa, nakha tɩɩ phuu fɛʋʋ Thãgba bɩɛl, dɛ bonɩ ji paarraalera hanɩ fãga too pa ƴɩɛra.
66008004	Dɩ latɩkoloolee isi gbɛbɩnanɛ tɩɩ phuusɔɔ Thãgba bɩɛl a the thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuulee nyɔ̃kɔɔ, dɩ ga-n jʋʋn Thãgbara.
66008005	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule gbaar latɩkolo 'wiidaale a ti bonɩ ji dɔɔ pɛr dɩɩ hi, dɩ dʋna faa thɩɩra, dɩ thãgba tiire kɔɔ hale na nɔ khena, na thãgba jʋ khor na thɩ jɩɩn.
66008006	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔɔkɛ fɔrɔnɩ tutuu makonyɔ kɔɔ gbɛbɩrɛ ʋ̃ ʋ̃ gbɛbɩrʋʋ.
66008007	Dɩ cacadaar kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dɩ thãgba bara hale na dɔɔ a nyanyaana tɔmɩn dɩ ga-n cʋr thɩɩra, dɩ thɩ phɛrɛ bɩɛl thɩ phɛrɛ yẽtherra kɔɔ hɩnɛ koo, dɩ thɩr der pa bɩɛl der paar yẽtherra kɔɔ hɩnɛ dakha, dɩ hɔ̃ ƴolosɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ hɩnɛ.
66008008	Dɩ balanyɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dɩ dɩkha gɩ, a ho gɔ̃gɔ̃ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, a do dɔ haar, a əl ji lanyʋɔnna, dɩ lanyɔ̃ phɛrɛ bɩɛl yẽtherra debi a do tɔmɩn.
66008009	Dɩ thɩ̃ tinə der pa bɩɛl der paar yẽtherra, kɛ hanɩ lanyʋɔnna a do yidara kɔɔ khiire, dɩ bato kɔ̃tĩ jɛ pa bɩɛl jɛ paar yẽtherra kɔɔ wɩɛlɛ fɛʋ.
66008010	Dɩ balãther thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dɩ ƴepələ̃bi kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ gɩ, a hana dɔɔ dɔlɩna khaa, a the ƴũ, a ji mɩɩr phɛrɛ bɩɛl mɩɩr phɛrɛ yẽtherra na yɔ bu kanasɔra.
66008011	Ƴepələ̃biree iilera n dʋɔn Dakhaa, dɩ yɔ ɓɛl bɩɛl yɔ kuur paar yẽtherra debire a khar kpakpakpa, dɩ tibil jɔjʋɔ kɔɔ khiire, dɩɩ do nyʋɔnɩlera debanɩ a khar dɔ nɔɔ.
66008012	Dɩ balanã thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dɩ thɩ̃ɛ kɔɔ cʋʋrɛ wi ɓɛl bɩɛl ɓɛl paar yẽtherra, na po ɓɛl bɩɛl daɓɛla yẽtherra, na ƴepələ̃bi der pa bɩɛl der paar yẽtherra, dɩ ga ɓɛlsɔɔle fɛʋ debire a birə, dɩ dɩwɩl ɓɛl bɩɛl ɓɛl paar yẽtherraa dahɩrɛ bure, mɛna gɩ ha dakha na dɩtɩnɛ.
66008013	Dɩ mɩ-n kɔɔ hɩɩnɛ a nɩɛ dɩ gbʋɔrɛ ubi da-n ka thãgbara ƴũ fii, sɩ da-n so nɔ khɩɩr ayɩ: Ga puurore, ga puurore, ga puure thɩdarara ɔbɔɔkɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu yẽtherɩkɛ sɛnɩ na ʋnɩ awɩ tutuu.
66009001	Dɩ balamɔɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ ƴepələ̃bireekɛ kɔɔ thɛnɩ ƴũ a ji thɩɩra, a 'lɛ thɛrɛ 'lee kõkor lakile.
66009002	Dɩ a gbaar a khɛrna thɛrɛ 'lee kõkorʋra, dɩ isiir the le dɩ ga-n jʋʋn a ho dɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ isiir, dɩ wire na jɩɛ birəre kõkor isiirraale.
66009003	Dɩ toosõosɔ kɔɔ ther isiirraale a bɩ̃bɩlã thɩɩra, dɩ wɩ kɔɔ 'lɛr punone dɩɩ mãkhana punoneekɛ lana thɩɩra n hananɩ.
66009004	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ so warɛ ayɩ, wa-n cʋʋ hʋɔn thɩɩra thɩ̃ɛ, dɩ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ phonɩ gɩ, dɩ thɩra ga, sɩ tɩbɩla dɩbara, kɛ na hananɩ Thãgbaa jẽ awɩ kobirə ga.
66009005	Wa kɔɔ 'lɛ hʋɛ a na kʋ tibilə', sɩ kpoore wa kpoo war a na cʋʋna pora yemɔɩ; dɩ kpooreekɛra wa kpoo warnɩ mɔ̃ laan n thanɩ tibil dɩ a-n khʋʋ, mɛ̃ ga ha.
66009006	Ga bɔɔle tιbιla na-n ƴaalɛ khir sι wa yι ga; khi thue na fʋ wɛr, sι khir na car sι na sι war.
66009007	Toosõosɔɔle hʋrɛ gãgʋʋsɔɔkɛ wι-n gbɛbιnι wι jalna kʋʋr. Wɩ subire thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ hɔnɩ dɛ fãgadaar kpɩɛr awɩ yʋɔ, sɩ awɩ ƴɛ ho tibil ƴɩɛ.
66009008	Wɩ hananɛ yʋsuune dɩɩ ho khɛraa yʋsũ, sɩ awɩ nyɩ̃ ho sidũ'ũ nyιma.
66009009	Dι wι hananɛ dakha kũkũ kɛɛdaa dιι ho thɛ dι wι kɛɛ, dι awι gbɛl n helle mɔ̃kɛ gãgo hotoro jɔjʋɔ n canι lõ kʋʋrra dι a-n tii.
66009010	Wι hananɛ sʋʋ dιι ho lã sʋʋ a hana tha paar cιba cιba, dι awι sʋraalera awι puno ha, kɛ wa-n cʋʋnanι tιbιla puure gι dana pora yemɔι.
66009011	Awι fãgadaarιkɛ dɔ warnι yʋʋ dʋɔn thɛrɛ 'lee kõkorʋʋ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu. Ɔɔ i na ebirə thιmιιr n dʋɔn Abadɔ̃, sι gιrɛkι thιmιιr wι-n wena Apolιyɔ̃; i kιrʋ dʋɔn gbõgolõdaar.
66009012	Caca puu 'lɛr kar, sι agιpι yenyɔ puu 'lɛr hale wo a na kpaan.
66009013	Dι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu maadõdaar kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dι ɩ̃ nιɛ nʋɔ dιι the dɛ bonι ji paar ʋma yenana, kɛ hanι Thãgbaa ƴɛra,
66009014	a so thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu maadõdaarraakɛ hananι tutuu ayι: Thʋba thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu yenãakɛ wι lini Efιratι mιιr kɔ̃tιιna a faa.
66009015	Dι wι kɔɔ thʋbιrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu yenãale kɛ gbɛbanι pι ga lιɛrraale, na ga wirəəle, na ga poraale, na ga yɛraale, wι kʋrɛ tibil der pa bιɛl der paar yẽtherra.
66009016	Dι awι sɔrasιsɔɔkɛ tɔɔnι gãgʋʋsɔra kɔɔ har gbιlanι der paar gbιlanι ɔɔ der pa taanyɔ. Thale mι kɔɔ nιɛ dι wι ha.
66009017	Ɩ̃ thɩ̃ nιrɔra thakɛ mι kɔɔ yι gãgʋʋsɔ na wɩrɛ jʋnɛ wɩnɩ dɩ wɩ ha: Wɩ kɔɔ hananɛ kũkũ kɛɛda sɩɛsɔ dɩɩ ho dɔɔ, na dathʋ̃phʋaasɔ, na dodaasɔɔkɛ hɔnɩ girbi. Sɩ gãgʋʋsɔɔ yʋʋle hor sidũ'ũ yʋʋ, sɩ dɔɔ na-n the awɩ nɔɔ, na isiir, na girbi.
66009018	Dɩ tibil der pa bɩɛl der paar yẽtherra kɔɔ khiire thɩlkena yẽtherraale kɛ dɔnɩ dɔɔ, na isiir, na girbi, kɛ n thɛnɩ gãgonaalee nɔɔ.
66009019	Gɩdonɩ gãgʋʋsɔɔlee puno, awɩ nɔra gɩ ha na awɩ sʋra. Awɩ sʋ hor siisɔ, a hana yʋʋ, dɩ gɛrra wɩ-n cʋʋna puurera.
66009020	Sι tibil ƴιrɛ sɛnι, kɛ thιlke caale na kʋna', wa-n debi haarrakɛ sι wι faa gιrɛ awι nyɛ̃ n cʋʋna', na mɔ̃ wι-n fʋɔrnι kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔa', na thιlaakɛ dɔnι dɛ na dɛ buloə', na thɛ na bokana ga, na thιra ga, kɛ na hananι yire dɩ wɩ yɩna ga, dɩ nũu gɩ dɩ wɩ nɩna ga, dɩ nɛɛ gɩ dɩ wɩ ɩɩrna ga.
66009021	Wa-n debi haar dakha sɩ wɩ faa awɩ tɩɩ kʋa', na awɩ sidumo thɩ̃ cʋa', na awɩ bɔdɛl cʋa', na awɩ yuə'.
66010001	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ yɩrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ wo kɛ hananɩ fãga dɩɩ və̃vĩə, dɩ the Thãgbaa dʋɔ da-n gbũ a paar ndɔlɔ̃paar, dɩ thãgba khalʋ hale ɔɔ yʋɔ, sɩ ɔɔ ƴɛ hor wire, dɩ ɔɔ nɛ ho dɔɔ.
66010002	A fʋrɔrɛ sɛbɛ buu dɩɩ phubi ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ, dɩ a sar lanyʋɔn na nyɔ̃bɔ nɔɔ, sɩ nyɔ̃bɩlã nɔɔ sa thɩɩ,
66010003	sɩ dɩ hulẽ nʋɔ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka a ho mɔ̃ sidũ'ũu n oornι. Ɔbɔɔkɛ a huleni thale thãgba phɛɛrɛ makonyɔ ther.
66010004	Ɔbɔɔkɛ thãgba phɛɛrɛ makonyɔɔle thenι pι, mι marra ɩ̃ khere sa nιɛ wire dιι the Thãgbaa dʋɔ ayι: Kpalanɛ na jιιn gιrɛ thãgba phɛɛrɛ makonyɔɔle kɔɔ sonι, sι fa-n khere ga.
66010005	Dι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛra mι kɔɔ yιnι dι jιιl lanyʋɔnna na thιιra, 'laarɛ nyɔ̃bɔ nyɔ̃ɔ thãgbara ƴũ,
66010006	sa ʋlfɛ da-n wena ʋrɛ dɔnι Yi hɩ̃daar bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorrι i, kɛ kɔɔ tenι ƴũ na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ha garnι, na thιι na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ha garnι, na lanyʋɔn na thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋʋkɛ ha garnι ayι: Pʋɔrɛ na hale bã;
66010007	sι bɔɔkɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔdaar na ʋnι ɔɔ tutuu, Thãgbaa thɩ̃ gbul na daan, mɔ̃kɛ a kɔɔ sonι ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔraakɛ dɔnι bobona.
66010008	Dι wireekɛ mι kɔɔ nιɛnι, kɛ thɛnι Thãgbaa dʋɔ, bire mιιna mι wo ayι: Jala, tea sɛbɛ buulera thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurəəkɛ jιlɛnι lanyʋɔnna na thιιra hananι ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ dιι phubi.
66010009	Dι mι jaal thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurəəle a sʋʋraa ayι, a ha mι sɛbɛ buurə. Dι a so marɛ ayι: Gba, khɔ. Ga kharrɛ wer afι bιnɔ, sι nɔɔ ga daarɛ a na ho thʋʋr.
66010010	Dι mι teere sɛbɛ buurə thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuu nyɔ̃kɔɔ a kho, dιι daar nɔɔ a ho thʋʋr, sι ɔbɔɔkɛ mι khonι pι, gι kha marɛ bιnɔ kpakpakpa.
66010011	Dι thιmιιr dã mɛr wo ayι: Dɔ fa n mιι gιrɛ Thãgba sonι, kɛ telenenι tιbιlasɔ, na caarsɔ, na thιmιιrsɔ, na fãgadaar jɔjʋɔ.
66011001	Dι mι kɔɔ 'lɛr jʋmũu dιι ho gbʋʋl, sa nɩ nʋɔ dɩɩ so mar ayɩ: Ɩrɛ, a mɩɛnɛ Thãgbaa cɔ hɩnɛ, na bonɩ ji paar, a therana wɩrɛ dɔnɩ fɔfɔraakɛ hanɩle.
66011002	Sɩ Thãgbaa cɔ phel gbaya wer, sɛ gar, fa-n mɩa', gɩdonɩ ca kpala wɩ ha, kɛ dɔnɩ wɩrɛ na kpɔ̃kpɔrɔnɛnɩ dɩ phuurə na nɛɛ na cʋʋna pora kpalanyɔ yenyɔ.
66011003	Ma har ɩ̃ sobɔ so jɩdara yenyɔɔkɛ tɔnɩ bɔrɔ kẽkena punone, dɩ wa mɩɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba sonɩ na cʋʋna wire gbιlanι na taanyɔ na kpalãther.
66011004	Wɛr dɔ olιvι thιra yenyɔ na dɔ carãa yenyɔ kɛ n jιlɛnι Kɔ̃tιnnaakɛ dɔnι thιιkɛɛ Kɔ̃tɩ̃.
66011005	Dι ado tibil ƴaal a cʋʋ wι puure, dɔɔ na ther awι nɔɔ na thii awι lãlaardara; dι ado tibil ƴaal a cʋʋ wɩ puure thalera wa kʋʋ ger.
66011006	Wι hananɛ punone a na khaanna ƴũ, dɩ thãgba nyʋɔn na ɩ̃ thɩɩra bɔɔkɛ wɩ hanɩ dɩ wa-n mɩɩ gɩrɛ Thãgba sona'. Wɩ hananɛ dakha punone a na debina nyʋɔn dɩ ga do tɔmɩn, a na gbana thɩlke lɩɩlɩɩ a na to thɩɩraakɛ bɔɔ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ-n ƴaalnɩ.
66011007	Ɔbɔɔkɛ wa mɩɩnɩ awɩ Thãgba thɩmɩɩle na pɩ, nʋmɩkɛ thɛnɩ thɛrɛ 'lee kõkorʋra na kena wɛr kʋʋr, a na kəə war, a na kʋ wɩ.
66011008	Sɩ awɩ for na phɩnɛ dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ kʋlã hʋ thɩ̃thɩɩn, kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ na sokpaa Sɔdɔm na Ejipiti, ka tɩbɩla kɔɔ kpanɩ dakha wɛrɩleraa Kɔ̃tɩ̃.
66011009	Tɩbɩla tɩbɩlaa thɩ̃thɩɩn, na caarra, na thιmιιrra, na ca kpalala, ιkhasɔ na hιιnɛ awι for na cʋʋna wire yẽther na dakuru, wa tu awι for n dɔ kaʋa'.
66011010	Dι awιdara na dor nɔɔ dι daʋ na kãkar na fʋlɛ tιbιla thιιra, wa-n thɔna kha khaardaasɔ bιɛlbιɛl, gιdonι Thãgbaa bobona yenyɔɔle kɔɔ kpoore tιbιlala thιιra.
66011011	A wire yẽther na dakuruule ka pι, fesueeke n 'laanɛnι yire, kɛ thɛnι Thãgbaa pa, lõ warɛ dι wι pal ιιr jιιl, dι ma kɔ̃tɩ̃ι fʋlɛlɛ wιrɛ kɔɔ yɛ wιnι.
66011012	Dɩ Thãgbaa bobona yenyɔɔle nɩrɛ nɔ khɩɩr dɩɩ the Thãgbaa dʋɔ ayɩ: Nɩ jʋnɛ kɛ. Dɩ wɩ jʋʋnɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ na ndɔlɔ̃paar, dɩ awɩ lãlaardara kɔɔ yɩ wɛr.
66011013	Ga bɔɔraalera thɩ jẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ, dɩ dɩ phɛrɛ bɩɛl dɩ phɛrɛ yʋɔrra kɔɔ jiire, dɩ tɩbɩla gbɩlanɩ makonyɔ kɔɔ khiire thɩ jɩɩnnaale, sɩ maar fʋlɛ wɩrɛ sɛnɩ ka, dɩ wa-n dʋbɩ Thãgba ire, kɛ hanɩ ƴũ.
66011014	Balanyɔ puu 'lɛr kar, sɩ hɩnɛ, balãtherdaa hale a na kpaan kɔrɔ.
66011015	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔdaar kɔɔ ʋnɛ ɔɔ tutuu, dɩ nɔ khena the Thãgbaa dʋɔ a so ayɩ: Fãgadaar dʋʋr thιιra koo, asι Kɔ̃tɩ̃ na ɔɔ Kirisiti hιna nɛnɛ̃ dιphã, dι ɔr na dɔ Fãgadaar bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ.
66011016	Dι kɔ̃tιna kpelẽ yenãale tɔɔnι Thãgbaa ƴɛra awι fãga too para gburõkure dɩ wa-n fʋɔr Thãgba,
66011017	ayɩ: Sɩ-n khɩɩ fɛr, fɛr Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar, kɛ hanɩle gɩrɛ, kɛ dakha kɔɔ hanɩle, gɩrɛraakɛ fɩ teenɩ afɩ fãga kɔ̃tɩ̃ a hɩ̃, a do gɩrɛ Fãgadaar.
66011018	Nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋrɛ tibil caar fɛʋ, sɩ afɩ nĩkhi wi phaan dɩ fa kɩɩlna gɩrɛ khe, sɩ na ka dakha afɩ thɔ̃dara Thãgbaa bobona na tɩɩ phuusɔ, na wɩrɛ n maannɩ afɩ i, tɩɩ mɔlɔ a gbana kɔ̃tɩna, sɩ dɩ fa-n kʋɛ wɩrɛra n kʋɛanɩ thɩɩ.
66011019	Dɩ Thãgbaa cɔ kɔɔ khɛrrɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩ ʋlfɛ khɛɛsʋʋ kɔɔ yɩrrɛ ɔɔ cɔrara, dɩ thãgba jʋ khor kɔɔ hale, na nɔ khena, na thãgba tiire, na thɩ jɩɩn, dɩ thãgba bar kɔ̃tɩna gbũgbũu na-n jɛ.
66012001	Dɩ jẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ yɩrrɛ thãgbara ƴũ, khɛr gɩ a to wire kẽkẽ khaa, sɩ por ha ɔɔ nɛ ballɔ, sa subi fãgadaar kpɩɛr dɩɩ hana ƴepələ̃be yʋɔr yenyɔ.
66012002	Dɩ khɛrra hananɛ pɛmɛr, dɩ mɔ̃ wallɛ fʋʋnɩ a jʋɔraa, a hulene ɔɔ bi kɔ̃ para.
66012003	Dɩ jẽ kpɩɩ bire yɩr wo le thãgbara ƴũ; gbakho sɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ gɩ a hana yʋʋ makonyɔ, na ʋma yʋɔr, sa subi fãga kpɛra makonyɔ ɔɔ yʋsɔrara.
66012004	Ɔɔ sʋ kɔɔ kpabɩrɛ ƴepələ̃bi der pa bɩɛl der paar yẽtherra le ƴũ, a der thɩɩra. Dɩ gbakhora jɩɩlɛ khɛrɩlee ƴɛra, kɛ ƴaalɛnɩ a kɔ̃ bi, ado a kʋɔn birə a gba a kho.
66012005	Dɩ khɛrra kʋɔn bɩsaan dɩ do kũubir, dɩɩ do ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ na-n khɛnɩ tibil caar fɛʋ na the gbʋʋl; sɩ wɩ vəən ɔɔ birə, a gba jʋʋnna ka Thãgba hanɩ na ka ɔɔ fãga too pa hanɩ.
66012006	Sɩ khɛr fʋʋ a jal bəənnə, ka dɔnɩ paarɩkɛ Thãgba gbɛbɩnɩ a thɩɩnʋʋ, dɩ mɛ̃ wa haanʋʋ wire gbɩlanɩ na taanyɔ na kpalãther.
66012007	Dɩ kʋʋr kɔɔ ɩɩrɛ le thãgbara ƴũ. Mɩsɛl na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔɔkɛ a doronɩ kɔ̃tɩn n kɔɔ kɛ̃kɛrɛna gbakhoolera, dɩ gbakhora na ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ kɔɔ kɛ̃kɛrɛna wɛr.
66012008	Sɩ gbakhora na puno wa', dɩ wa yɩ too paar le ƴũ bã.
66012009	Dɩ wɩ tinəne gbakho kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle, kɛ dɔnɩ si tɩ̃ɩ, kɛ wɩ-n wenɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃, kɛ n dɔnɩ dakha Satã, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛra n fɩlɛnɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ thɩɩra, wɩ tinəəne a weguu faa thɩɩra, mɔ̃ wɩ tinəəni mɛ̃ wɩ tinə ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thusɔ.
66012010	Dɩ mɩ nɩrɛ nɔ khɩɩr dɩɩ the Thãgbaa dʋɔ a so ayɩ: Nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã asɩ Thãgbaa taa daan, na ɔɔ fãga, na ɔɔ fãgadaar do, na ɔɔ Kirisitii puno hana, gɩdonɩ omɩnaa so pɛdaarra, kɛ dɔnɩ ʋrɛ n kɔɔ pɛ warnɩ sor dɩwɩlʋ na dɩtɩnɛ Thãgbaa ƴɛra, a kɔɔ tinəəne a weguu faa.
66012011	Sɩ asɩ omisɔ kɔɔ punoone dɩɩ do Bana bii tɔmɩna gɩ the, na awɩ sobɔ so jɩ thɩmɩɩra; wa kɔɔ na awɩ yi sa ma khirə'.
66012012	Gɛr gɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ na kãkanɛ, na nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ harɔnɩ, sɩ ga puure thɩɩra na lanyʋɔnna, gɩdonɩ Satã gbune anɩ pa, nĩkhii fʋʋrɛ jɔɔ ka, gɩdonɩ a jɩrɛ dɩ bɔɔ fɩɩʋ sɩɛ dɩbara.
66012013	Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ gbakhora yɩɛnι dιι do wι tinəəne a wee faa thιιra, a ιιrɛ̃ da-n wee khɛrιlera kɔnanι kũubirile.
66012014	Dι khɛrιle 'lɛ gbʋɔr gbɛl kɔ̃tιna yenyɔ, dι mɛ̃ a na ubinə a na jal bəənnə ka dɔnι ɔɔ pa, ka wa-n haanʋʋnι gι cʋʋna yɛna yẽther na dakuru, a hʋnɔna siilera.
66012015	Sι siile kɔɔ cιrrɛ nyʋɔn ɔɔ nɔra dιι ho mιιr, dι ga-n kpaan khɛrraale gι halʋʋ gι kpɛɛ nyʋɔnɔ.
66012016	Sι thιι kɔɔ taarɛ khɛrιle a ha nʋɔ a dιι nyʋɔnna gbakho cιrnι dιι do mιιr.
66012017	Dι nĩkhii kɔɔ fʋrɛ gbakhoole ka khɛrraale, dι a gbaar jal da-n ke kʋʋr na khɛrι məlikɛ sɛnι, kɛ dɔnι wιrɛ n hιnɛnι Thãgbaa jɔfʋ, kɛ fɔrɔnι sobɔrιkɛ Jeju kɔɔ mιιnι.
66012018	Sι lanyɔ̃ gbalãkothιnna gbakhoole jιιl.
66013001	Agιpι mι kɔɔ yιrɛ nʋm dι ιιr lanyʋɔnna da-n jʋʋn, a hana ʋma yʋɔr na yʋʋ makonyɔ, dι fãgadaar kpɛra yʋɔr hale ɔɔ ʋ̃sɔrara, dι i kʋɛ thιmιιr hale ɔɔ yʋsɔrara dakha.
66013002	Dι nʋmιlera mι yιnι a-n honanɛ kpe, sι ɔɔ nɛ na-n hona sιɓɛlɛ̃ nɛɛ, sι ɔɔ gbuokhu ho sidũ'ũ gbuokho. Dι gbakhoolera kɔɔ haarɛ ɔɔ fãga, na ɔɔ fãga too pa, na punone dιι kɔ̃tĩ ka.
66013003	Dι mι yιrɛ ɔɔ yʋsɔɔlera bιɛl dιι ho tɔmĩ sɛ khoo a 'lɛ, kɛ dɔnι khikhi khoo. Sι ɔɔ khikhi khoolera kɔɔ kpɛɛrɛ. Dι tιbιla thιιra koo n kɔɔ kpar nʋmιnaale na nɔ kpaarɛ.
66013004	Dι wι-n gburõkure gbakhoraale gιdonι a kɔɔ har nʋmιle ɔɔ puno. Dι mɛ̃ wι-n gburõku nʋmιnaalera dι wa-n sona ayι: Amɛ hale a ho nʋmιle, dι amɛ na punone a na kɛ̃kɛrɛnaa?
66013005	Dι nʋmιle 'lɛr hʋɛ da-n sona kuune, da-n mιιna dakha i kʋɛ thιmιa, a 'lɛr punone a na-n cʋʋna thĩɛ pora kpalanyɔ yenyɔ.
66013006	Dι a har ɔɔ nɔra da-n kpɛna Thãgba, da-n kʋɛna ɔɔ i, da-n sʋʋrna Thãgbaa pa na wιrɛ hanι Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
66013007	A kɔɔ 'lɛr hʋɛ a kena tιι phuusɔ kʋʋr a puno wi, a 'lɛr dakha punone caarra fɛʋ, na tιbιlala fɛʋ, na thιmιιrra fɛʋ, na ca kpalala fɛʋ.
66013008	Dι tιbιla fɛʋ thιιra n gburõkuraarɛ, kɛ dɔnι wιrɛ awι i na kherenι yi sɛbɛraakɛ dɔnι Bana biida ga, kɛ dɔnι ʋrɛ wι kɔɔ kʋnι sι thιιkɛ na kɔɔ ti pa'.
66013009	Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananι nũu, dɔ a na-n nιɛ.
66013010	Ʋrɛɛkɛ ga teenanι a dɔ dee, deera a na do; dι ʋrɛɛkɛ n kɔnι tibil na bajιna, bajιnana wa kʋnaa phubi. Gιrɛɛkɛra tιι phuusɔ na nιna awι ha fʋ na awι ha pɛ.
66013011	Agιpι mι kɔɔ yιrɛ nʋ̃ kpιι wo da-n the thιιra, a hana ʋma yenyɔ dιι ho Bana biida, sι da-n mιι gbakhoo kha.
66013012	Dι a hananɛ caca nʋmι fãgara da-n dona thɔma ɔɔ ƴɛra; dι a cʋʋrɛ thιι na wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ harɔnι dɩ wa-n gburõku caca nʋmɩnaale, kɛ kɔɔ hananɩ tɔmɩ̃ sɛ khookɛ dɔnɩ khikhi khoo, sɩ dɩɩ kpɛɛ.
66013013	Dɩ a n cʋʋrɛ nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ kɔ̃tɩna, dɩ ba cʋʋnanakɛ dɔɔ dιι the ƴũ a na ji thιιra dι tιbιla fɛʋ na-n yιɛ.
66013014	Dι nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔɔlera a kɔɔ 'lɛnι hʋɛ a na-n cʋʋ caca nʋmɩ ƴɛrara, gɛr a-n fɩɩlna tɩbɩla thɩɩra da-n so war dɩ yɩ, wɩ cʋɛ nʋmɩlera thɩl khaa gbelẽ gbelẽ, kɛ dɔnɩ nʋmɩkɛra wɩ kɔɔ cɩnɩ na bajɩna sɩ dɩ le.
66013015	Balanyɔ nʋmɩle 'lɛr punone da-n 'laana fesue thɩɛnaalera wɩ cʋʋnɩ dɩ ho caca nʋmna, dɩ mɛ̃ thɩ̃ɛɛlera wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ dɩ ho nʋm n mɩɩ nʋɔ, da-n kʋʋrna dakha wɩrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ na-n gburõkuneni thɩɛnaalera wɩ cʋʋnɩ dɩ ho nʋma'.
66013016	Dɩ a cʋʋrɛ tɩbɩla fɛʋ tɩɩ mɔlɔ a gbana kɔ̃tɩna, lɛ̃lɛ na bɔdara, waɩa na dea, wɩ pɛ war jɩɩn awɩ nyɔ̃bɔsɔra, na awɩ kobisɔra.
66013017	Dɩ tibil bɩɛllakɛ na puno na the thɩ̃ɛ, agɩbo a dolõ thɩ̃ɛ, sɩɩ do aa hana jɩɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ nʋmɩlee i agɩbo ɔɔ i nɩmɔrɔaa ga.
66013018	Kɩɛr dʋɔn kpɛsɛ nɩna paar. Ʋrɛɛkɛ hananɩ yʋʋ a thera a jɛ nʋmɩlee nɩmɔrɔ kɩr, gɩdonɩ tibil nɩmɔrɔ gɩ, dɩ ga nɩmɔrɔ har taa maadõ na kpalãther maadõ.
66014001	Dɩ ma hɩɩn dɩɩ do Bana bii gɩ, a jɩɩl Sɩyɔ̃ gɔ̃gʋɔna, dɩ tɩbɩla gbɩlanɩ tamaa na kpalanyɔ na gbɩlanɩ yenã ha kha na ɔr, dɩ ɔɔ i na ɔɔ Thɩɩ i khere awɩ kobisɔra.
66014002	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ nɩrɛ wire dɩɩ the Thãgbaa dʋɔ a ho yɔ jɔjʋɔ n hela, dɩ ga-n hona dakha thãgba phɛɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, dɩ wireelera mɩ nɩɛnɩ gɩ hor salã bɩ̃dara wɛ dɩ wa-n bɩ̃ salãa.
66014003	Dɩ wɩ-n khɩnɛ nɩ phaa fãga too pa ƴɩɛra, na thɩ̃ ye yenã na kɔ̃tɩnasɔɔ ƴɛra. Dɩ tibil na hale a na puno nɩɛɛlera a na dɩɩr, saagado tɩbɩla gbɩlanɩ tamaa na kpalanyɔ na gbɩlanɩ yenãale Thãgba kɔɔ birseni thɩɩraakɛ gaaga.
66014004	Wɛr dɔ wɛkɛ na kɔɔ biseneni dɩbara na khɛra ga, gɩdonɩ wa kɔɔ phɩna khɛrrakɛ a yɩ ga, dɩ wɛrra n kpaanɛ Bana biirə paar fɛʋʋkɛ a-n jalnι. Wɛr dɔ wɩrɛ Thãgba kɔɔ tini tɩbɩlala, a birse wɩ do caca tɩbɩla Thãgbara na Bana biirə.
