66014005	Dɩ awɩ nɔra sõso thɩmɩɩ bɩɛllakɛ na kɔɔ the la', wɛr dɔ tɩbɩlaakɛ na hananɩ dɩ paara'.
66014006	Dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ wo dɩ ubi da-n ka thãgbara ƴũ fĩi, a hana tutugo bʋɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ khorrdaa a na-n mɩɩ tɩbɩla thɩɩra, na ca kpalala fɛʋ, na caarra fɛʋ, na thɩmɩɩrra fɛʋ, na tɩbɩlala fɛʋ;
66014007	sɩ nɔ khɩɩr a-n mɩɩna da-n so ayɩ: Na-n ma Thãgba, na-n dʋba ɔɔ i, gɩdonɩ bɔɔkɛ a na kɩɩlnanɩ tɩbɩla gɩ daan. Na-n kpãganɛ ɔrkɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ ƴũ, na thɩɩ, na lanyʋɔn, na yɔ bu kanasɔ fɛʋ.
66014008	Dɩ balanyɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ kpaan da-n so ayɩ: Babɩlɔn dɩ kʋkʋʋra jire, a jire pɩ, ɔrkɛra kɔɔ cʋɛnɩ tibil caar fɛʋ dɩ wɩ yɔ ɔɔ bɔdɛl ta kha kpakpakpa.
66014009	Dɩ balãther thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ kpaan da-n sona nɔ khɩɩr ayɩ: Ado tibil na gburõku nʋmɩnaale na gɩrɛ wɩ cʋʋnɩ dɩ ga-n hʋʋ, a 'lɛna dakha ɔɔ jẽ kobiro na nyɔɔna,
66014010	ntɛ na yɔr dakha taanɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa nĩkhida, kɛ dɔnɩ ta khaa kpakpakpa, kɛ a pɛrnɩ ɔɔ nyɔ̃kpona sɩ dɩkha na nyanyaanɔa', dɩ a na 'wãgarɛ dɔɔra na girbi thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu phuusɔɔ ƴɛra na Bana bii ƴɛra.
66014011	Dɩ awɩ 'wãga isi baan dɩ ga-n jʋʋn bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ. Hιιrɛ na hale kpιιrakɛ dιwιlʋ na dιtιnɛ wιrɛraakɛ n gburõkuneni nʋmιnaale na thιɛnaakɛ wι cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ hʋa', na tibil wo tibilləəkɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnɩ ɔɔ i jã'.
66014012	Gɩrɛɛkɛra tɩɩ phuusɔɔkɛ n hɩnɛnɩ Thãgbaa jɔfʋ, a hanana ha pɛrɛ Jejura, na nɩna awɩ ha fʋ.
66014013	Dɩ mɩ nɩrɛ nʋɔ dɩɩ the Thãgbaa dʋɔ ayɩ: Khera gɩrɛra: Nɛnɛ̃ bɔɔkɛ dɩphã ga-n dar wɛkɛra n khenɩ mɔ̃ wɩ donɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩda; dɩ Thu Phuu dee aa: Ɔɔ sobɔr gɩ, wɩ thʋ̃ wɩ hɩɩrrakɛ awɩ thɔ̃ khe dorara mɛ̃, gɩdonɩ awɩ thɔ̃ɔkɛ wɩ kɔɔ cʋʋnɩ 'lor nɛɛ dɩ ga-n kpa war.
66014014	Dɩ ma hɩɩn dɩɩ do ndɔlɔ̃pa bulo gɩ, dɩ tibil hale a too ndɔlɔ̃paarrara a ho tibili bikuun, a subi dɛ fãgadaar kpɩɛr, sa fʋrɔ hɔ̃ khabɩda khɩɩ ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
66014015	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ ther Thãgbaa cɔ a hulẽ dɩɩ khɩɩr ka olela tɔɔnɩ ndɔlɔ̃paarra ayɩ aa: Laanɛ afɩ hɔ̃ khabɩdara a na khaba jɔ, gɩdonɩ jʋ kha bɔɔ daan, dɩ thɩɩra daan khar jʋ khaa.
66014016	Dɩ olera tɔɔnɩ ndɔlɔ̃paarra 'laarɛ ɔɔ hɔ̃ khabɩda thɩɩra dɩ ga-n khabɩ thɩɩ jʋ khaa.
66014017	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ ther Thãgbaa cɔɔkɛ hanɩ Thãgbaa dʋɔ, a fʋrɔ dakha hɔ̃ khabɩda khɩɩ.
66014018	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpɩɩ wo, kɛ hananɩ punone dɔɔra, the bonɩ ji paar, a so nɔ khɩɩr olela hananɩ hɔ̃ khabɩda khɩɩle ayɩ: 'Laanɛ afɩ hɔ̃ khabɩda khera, a kurona dɩvɛ̃ thɩr beele sɛnɩ jɩrkpɩrɩɩ, kɛ hanɩ thɩɩra, gɩdonɩ bera bɩnɛ.
66014019	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thurə 'laa ɔɔ hɔ̃ khabɩdara thɩɩra dɩɩ kuur dɩvɛ̃ thɩr bera thɩɩra, dɩ gba a dʋna Thãgbaa nĩkhi bi nã pa kɔ̃tɩ̃.
66014020	Dɩ wɩ kɔɔ naan beelera le bi nã paar dɩ khuirə, dɩ bi nã paarra tɔmɩn ther le, a deer a jal dã kilə tãather, gɩ jʋʋnɛ dakha a dã gãgʋʋ gbã.
66015001	Agɩpɩ dɩ ɩ̃ yɩ jẽ kpɩɩ wo Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ka a kpaa nʋɔ; thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔ wɛ a fʋrɔ thɩlkena makonyɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ pɩpɩɩdaa, gɩdonɩ gɛr na cʋɛ Thãgbaa nĩkhi dɩ ga pɩɩr waa vʋ̃ʋ.
66015002	Dɩ mɩ yɩrɛ thɩ̃ɛ dɩɩ ho lanyʋɔnɩkɛ hɔnɩ hɩɩnʋ, dɩɩ nyanyaana dɔɔ, a yɩna dakha wɩrɛ kɔɔ punoneni nʋmɩle na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ wɩ cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ hʋʋ, na ɔɔ nɩmɔrɔ i, dɩ wɩ jɩɩl lanyʋɔnnaalera hɔnɩ hɩɩnʋ, sa fʋrɔ Thãgbaa salã,
66015003	sɩ dɩ wa-n khɩ̃ Mʋɩjɩɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaa thɔ̃daarɩ nɩ, na Bana bii nɩ, dɩ wa-n sona ayɩ: Afɩ thɩ̃ cʋʋ kɔ̃tɩnɛ a kpaa nʋɔ ya Kɔ̃tɩn, Thãgba fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar; afɩ hʋsɔ sarrɛ a do sobɔr, fɛr caar fɛʋʋ Fãgadaar.
66015004	Ʋmɔ̃ na bɔ fɛr Kɔ̃tɩn maar na afɩ i cʋʋr? Gɩdonɩ fɛr bɩɛl dɩbara pho, dɩ tibil caar fɛʋ na ɩnɛ na gburõku far ƴɛ thɩ̃thɩɩn, gɩdonɩ afɩ fɩl sar thɔ̃ yɩrrɛ dɩphã.
66015005	A gele pɩ, ma hɩɩnɛ a yɩ Thãgbaa cɔ kãkɛ kẽkẽ waa hanɩ, dɩ Thãgba harɔ dɩ ga-n khɛr le Thãgbaa dʋɔ.
66015006	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔɔkɛ fɔrɔnɩ thɩlkena makonyɔ ther Thãgbaa cɔ, a to kẽkẽ bulona dɩ a-n carbara, sa khɩmɩ dɛ lophɛrɛ kũkuno.
66015007	Dɩ thɩ̃ ye yenãale bɩɛl har thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔɔle dɛ bilẽse makonyɔ, dɩɩ hinə Thãgbaakɛ hananɩ yire bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorrɩ nĩkhi.
66015008	Dɩ Thãgbaa cɔ kɔɔ hinəne isiirikɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa i dʋbɩra na ɔɔ puno hanana, dɩ ga do tibil bɩɛllakɛ na punone a na lõ Thãgbaa cɔa', phaphapha thɩlkena makonyɔɔle thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔ fʋrɔnɩ n pɩɩr wɩbɩ.
66016001	Dɩ mɩ nɩrɛ nɔ khɩɩr dɩɩ the Thãgbaa cɔ, a so thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔraale ayɩ: Nɩ jala na deere thɩɩra bilẽse makonyɔɔle hananɩ Thãgbaa nĩkhi.
66016002	Dɩ cacadaar jaal a deer ɔɔ bilẽsi thɩɩra, dɩ nɔr kpal dɩkhaakɛ n helanɩ fʋlɛ tɩbɩlaakɛ hananɩ nʋmɩlee jẽ, dɩ wa-n fʋɔrna thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ wɩ cʋʋnɩ dɩɩ hʋʋ.
66016003	Dɩ balanyɔdaar deer ɔɔ bilẽsi lanyʋɔnna, dɩɩ debi a ho tɔmɩnɩkɛ n ƴɔnɩ khirera, dɩ thɩ̃ ye fɛʋʋkɛ hanɩ lanyʋɔnna khiire.
66016004	Dɩ balãtherdaar deer ɔɔ bilẽsi mɩɩrra na yɔ bu kanana, dɩɩ debi a do tɔmɩn.
66016005	Le mɩ nɩɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ dɔnɩ yɔdaar da-n so ayɩ: Fɛr Tɩɩ phuu, kɛ hanɩle gɩrɛ, kɛ kɔɔ hanɩle, fɩ sarrɛ kɩɩlɛlaakɛ fɩ kɩɩlnɩ;
66016006	gɩdonɩ wɩ kɔɔ deere tɩɩ phuusɔɔ tɔmɩ̃, na Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ tɔmɩ̃, dɩ nɛnɛ̃ dɩphã fɩ ha wɛr dakha tɔmɩnna wɩ yɔ, gɩdonɩ gɛr wɩ teena.
66016007	Dɩ ɩ̃ nɩɛ bonɩ ji paar dɩɩ so aa: Ɔɔ Kɔ̃tɩn, Thãgba fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar, afɩ kɩɩlsɔra sarrɛ gɩ dor dakha sobɔr.
66016008	Dɩ balanãdaar deer ɔɔ bilẽsi wirera, dɩ wire 'lɛr punone a thii tɩbɩla na dɔɔ.
66016009	Dɩ daphʋɛ kpõkpõkpõ kɔɔ thiire tɩbɩla, sɩ wa-n debi haar wɩ dʋbɩ Thãgbaa iə', sɩ wɩ-n kpɛr Thãgbaakɛ hananɩ punone thɩlke caarsɔraale.
66016010	Dɩ balamɔɩdaar deer ɔɔ bilẽsi nʋmɩ fãga too para, dɩ ɔɔ fãga dɩ birəre, dɩ tɩbɩla na-n dʋɔn nɔfaar khooraakɛ gɩ-n kho wɩnɩ.
66016011	Sɩ wa-n debi haar sɩ wɩ faa awɩ thɔ̃ cʋʋra ga, sι wι-n kpɛr Thãgbaakɛ hanιle ƴũ hellelaakɛ gι-n hel wιnɩ, na awι nɔrraakɛ wι hananι.
66016012	Dι maadõdaar deer ɔɔ bilẽsi Efιratι mιιr kɔ̃tιιna, dι ɔɔ nyɔ̃ ι fɛʋ, dι mɛ̃ hʋɛ na har dι fãgadara na the wi phã paar na ɩ̃.
66016013	Dι ɩ̃ yι kɔ̃tɛɛbi hɔ̃hɔla yẽther, dι wι ho sιbɔna, bιɛl na-n the gbakhoo nɔra, bιɛl na-n the nʋmιlee nɔra, bιɛl na-n the sõso bobonιlee nɔra.
66016014	Gιdonι wɛr dʋɔn kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔkɛ n cʋɛnι nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛsɔ, kɛ n jalanι fãgadarasɔra thιιraakɛ fɛʋ, dι wι kpa wι a gbɛbιrι kʋʋrraakɛ na hanɩ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daarɩ wi kɔ̃tɩna.
66016015	Hɩnɛ, ma ɩnɛ yudaar khaa. Ga dar ʋrɛraakɛ n jʋrɛnɩ da-n jɩɩ hɩɩnna dakha ɔɔ kẽkẽsɔ, dɩ mɛ̃ a na-n ɩɩrna sãɓɔlɔ̃ gɩ ba phuroo yicuru n fʋʋa'.
66016016	Dɩ kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔle kpa wɛr a gbɛbɩ paarɩkɛ wɩ-n wenɩ na ebirə thɩmɩɩr: Armagedɔ̃.
66016017	Dɩ makonyɔdaar deer ɔɔ bilẽsi jɩɛra, dɩ nɔ khɩɩr the Thãgbaa cɔ, le ƴũ fãga too paarra, a so ayɩ: Gɩ daan mɛ̃.
66016018	Dɩ thãgba jʋ khor, na nɔ khena, na thãgba tiire, na thɩ jẽ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ ka kɔɔ hale. Thɩ jɩɩn thale na kɔɔ hale kɛkɛra tɩbɩla kɔɔ thenɩ dɩɩra ga, gɩ thʋnɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ka.
66016019	Dɩ dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ tɩnɛ tɩnɛ paar yẽther, dɩ tibil caar fɛʋʋ dɩsɔ kɔɔ jiire, dɩ thãgba jɩnanɛ Babɩlɔn dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩle a haa nyɔ̃kpʋʋnɩkɛ ɔɔ nĩkhi khe tã hironi a yɔ.
66016020	Dɩ yɔ dɩɩsɔ fɛʋ kɔɔ fuulele, dɩ gɔ̃gɔna na ha yɩrra bã.
66016021	Dɩ thãgba bar kɔ̃tɩna gbũgbũu, kɛ bɩɛlɩ dʋbɩ mãkhananɩ nã kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ dʋbɩ, the ƴũ dɩ ga-n bɩɩr tɩbɩla, dɩ tɩbɩla n kpɛr Thãgba thɩlkɩɩrraale dɔnɩ thãgba bara, gɩdonɩ thɩlkɩɩrɩle thʋnɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ ka.
66017001	Agɩpɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl makonyɔraale fʋrɔnɛnɩ bilẽse makonyɔ pɔr, a so mar ayɩ: Ɩna kɛ, ma nɩ farɛ khɛ bɔdɛl kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩlee kɩɩl, kɛ tɔɔnɩ yɔ jɔjɔ nʋɔra.
66017002	Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛra fãgadara thɩɩra n cʋʋrɔnι bɔdɛl thɔma, dι tιbιla thιιra yɔr ɔɔ bɔdɛl tã dι ga-n kʋ wι.
66017003	Dιι do Thu Phuu gι a gba mι a jalna bəənnə, dι le mι yι khɛr dι too nʋ̃ sιɛra kpakpakpa, dι i kpɛ thιmιιr haar khere ɔɔ tomιra koo, sι dι hana yʋʋ makonyɔ na ʋma yʋɔr.
66017004	Khɛrra tor kẽkẽ sιɛ himə himə, na kẽkẽ sιɛ kpakpakpa, sa gba dɛ, na boka the nɔ khena, na lẽbii a gbɛbιna biire. Dι khɛrra hananɛ dɛ bilẽsire a fʋrɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ, dιι hinə kpɔ̃kpɔrɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ na thɩ̃ biseekɛ dɔnι ɔɔ bɔdɛl cʋʋ thɩ̃.
66017005	Dι ire hale a khere ɔɔ kobirə sa do i gbul ayι: Babιlɔn dι kʋkʋʋra, bɔdɛlasɔ na thιιkɛɛ kpɔ̃kpɔrɔ̃ thɩ̃ι nι gι.
66017006	Dι mι yιrɛ khɛrra dι yɔ tιι phuusɔɔ tɔmɩ̃, na wιrɛ wι kʋʋrnι Jejuu soraa tɔmɩ̃, dι ga-n kʋʋ. Ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ kɔɔ yɩɩnɩ, nʋɔ kɔɔ kpaa mɛr dɩɩ pho ka.
66017007	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bule mi aa: Mɔ̃gɩdo dɩ nʋɔ kpaa fɩ? Ma mɩɛ fɛr thɩ̃ gbulikɛ dɔnɩ khɛrɩdaalera na nʋmɩle a tooronɩɩda, kɛ hananɩ yʋʋ makonyɔ na ʋma yʋɔr.
66017008	Nʋmɩle fɩ kɔɔ yɩnɩ dɩ kɔɔ hale, sɩ aa hale nɛnɛ̃ bã, a na ther thɛrɛ 'lee kõkorʋra, a na jal bu paar, dɩ tɩbɩlaakɛ hanɩ thɩɩra, kɛ awɩ i na kɔɔ kherenɩ yi sɛbɛra sɩ dɩ thɩɩkɛ tə', nʋɔ na kpaa wɛr mɔ̃ wa yɩnɩ nʋmɩle, gɩdonɩ a kɔɔ hale, sɩ aa hale nɛnɛ̃ bã, sɩ dɩɩ do a na bire na ɩɩr wo.
66017009	Kɩɛr dʋɔn yʋ bʋɔ na kpɛsɛ nɩna paar. Yʋʋ makonyɔɔle dʋɔn gɔ̃gɔna makonyɔɔkɛ khɛrra tooronɩ.
66017010	Fãgadara makonyɔ gɩ nɩna dakha. Yemɔɩ kɔɔ jire, sɩ bɩɛl bo jɩɩl, sɩ bɩɛl hale aa ɩ̃ pa'. Sɩ ado a ɩ̃, bɔɔ gbe teana a tɔɔ.
66017011	Nʋmɩkɛ kɔɔ hanɩle sɩ aa hale bã, ɔr thɛthɛra dʋɔn fãgadaarɩkɛ dʋɔnnɩ makõtherdaar, ɔrra dɔ dakha bɩɛl makonyɔdarara, sɩ bu paar a-n jal thale.
66017012	Ʋma yʋɔrɩkɛ fɩ yɩnɩ dʋɔn fãgadara yʋɔr, sɩ wa fʋ awɩ fãgadaar thɔ̃ pa', sɩ wɩ 'lɛr fãga wer, a na do fãgadara lɩɛr bɩɛl na nʋmɩle.
66017013	Kpɩɛr bɩɛl wɩ hana dɩ wa gbaar awɩ fãga na awɩ puno a na ha nʋmɩle.
66017014	Wa kɛ̃kɛrɛnanɛ Bana bii, sɩ Bana bii na puno wer gɩdonɩ ɔr dʋɔn Kɔ̃tɩ̃ kpɩɛ kɔ̃tɩnana, na Fãgadaar kpɩɛ fãgadarara, dɩ wɩrɛ Thãgba wenɩ, kɛ a phiirni, kɛ dʋɔraanɩ sobɔ tɩbɩlaakɛ hanaanɩ kha, na puno wer dakha.
66017015	Dɩ a so marɛ ayɩ: Nyʋɔnsɔɔkɛ fɩ yɩnɩ, dɩ khɛ bɔdɛlɩle tooro, tɩbɩla wɛ, na tibil jɔ bərəəm, na tibil caarsɔ, na thɩmɩɩ caarsɔ.
66017016	Dɩ ʋma yʋɔrɩle fɩ yɩnɩ na nʋmɩle, wa laarɛ khɛ bɔdɛlɩle, a na phʋʋnʋʋ sι na sιιraa da toona sãɓɔlɔ̃; wa khor ɔɔ nʋ̃ wa hιιnɛ dakha dɔɔra.
66017017	Gιdonι Thãgba pιɛr awι hara wι cʋɛ thĩɛɛle gι ha mɔ̃kɛ ιnɛr Thãgba n ƴaalnι, wι cʋɛ dakha thɩ̃ɛɛle na kpιɛr bιɛl, a gba awι fãgadaar do a hana nʋmιle phaphapha Thãgbaa thιmιι n dã gι ha oti.
66017018	Sι khɛrιle fι yιnι, ɔr dɔ dι kɔ̃tɩ̃ιkɛ hananι fãga fãgadarara thιιra.
66018001	A gele pι, ma hιιnɛ a yι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu kpιιkɛ hananι punone jɔɔ ka, dι the Thãgbaa dʋɔ da-n gbũ, dι ɔɔ carbara hιrɛ thιι.
66018002	Dι a hulene nʋɔ dιι khιιr ka ayι: A jire, a jire, Babιlɔn dι kɔ̃tιιna jire. Gι debire a do kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ cɔ pa mɛ̃, na kɔ̃tɛɛbi puunə fɛʋʋ wɔ̃ pa, na 'lominə fɛʋʋkɛ biseneni dι tιbιla na-n laarι wɔ̃ pa.
66018003	Gιdonι tibil caar fɛʋ kɔɔ yɔr ɔɔ bɔdɛl tãakɛ n ιnananι Thãgbaa nĩkhi. Ɔr dɔ ʋrɛ fãgadara thιιra kɔɔ cʋʋrɔnι bɔdɛl thɔma, dι dakha ƴaƴaba thιιra debire a do lẽledara dιι do ɔɔ nũfe thɩ̃ ƴaal jɔɔ dɔ nɔɔ.
66018004	Dι ɩ̃ nι wi kpιι wo dιι the Thãgbaa dʋɔ a so ayι: Ɩ̃ too wei, nι thɛ ɔɔ pa, a mɛ̃ gaa ga hor na lʋʋn ɔɔ sopugorara nι ba 'lɛ thιlkιιrιkɛ teleneenι.
66018005	Gιdonι ɔɔ sopugosɔra thʋnɛ cõcool waa a ba dã Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dι Thãgba jιnanɛ ɔɔ thɩ̃ gõgolõsɔ.
66018006	Nι lιmaa mɔna a kɔɔ lιmιnι, nι birə birsene balanyɔ a hanaa mɔna ɔɔ thɔ̃ hanι; nyɔ̃kpõ ʋrɛra a kɔɔ deernanι a 'laa, nι birə mιɛna wa nyɔ̃kpona balanyɔ a hanaa.
66018007	Mɔ̃kɛra a-n kɔɔ kanι ire a hanana nũfe thɩ̃ɛ jɔɔ, nι hanaa ɔmɛna 'wãgarɛ na nιwɛ. Gɩdonɩ a-n sor le ɔɔ hara dɩ yɩ aa, khɛ nũfe toore ɩnɩ too aa, ga do khikhɛrʋ ɩnɩ doa', ɩna yɩ bɩwɛ kpɩɩraka'.
66018008	Dɩ gɛrra na dɔ nɔɔ wi bɩɛl 'lẽ'lẽ'lẽ dɩbara thɩlkenaakɛ dɔnɩ kho puunə, na bɩwɛ, na kɔmɛr na daanɛ, dɔɔ na hɩnaa dakha; gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaakɛ n kɩlɛnaanɩ, aa hana fãga kpãkpalã ga.
66018009	Fãgadara fɛʋ thɩɩraakɛ kɔɔ cʋɛnaanɩ bɔdɛl thɔma, a mʋʋnaa kha nũfe thɩɛna, wa khɩɩrɛ wa-n bɩna ɔɔdarara ɔbɔɔkɛ wa yɩnɩ isiirikɛ n thɛnɩ ɔɔ hɩna.
66018010	Ƴɔɔ wa jɩɩl maar n fʋlɛ wɩ ɔɔ 'wãgara, dɩ wa sor nayɩ: Gɩ puurore, gɩ puure Babɩlɔn dɩ kɔ̃tɩɩnana, dι kʋkʋʋ thakɛ sι dιι do lιɛr bιɛl dapaara afι kιιl dã fɛr.
66018011	Dι ƴaƴaba thιιra khιιrɛ dι wa-n bιna ɔɔdara, gιdonι tibil na-n the wι thɩ̃ɛsɔ bã,
66018012	kɛ dɔnι thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ wι cʋʋnanɩ dɛ, na dɛ bulosɔ, na boka ƴɩrɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ, na lẽbiisɔ, na kẽkẽ ɓɔna, na kẽkẽ sɛna himə himə, na kẽkẽ hɩlʋsɔ, na kẽkẽ sɛna kpakpakpa, na thɩr caarsɔɔkɛ n nɛnɩ yɩrra, na thɩr ƴɩrɛ wɩ cʋʋnanɩ thũgbu khɛla, na thɩr khena, na the sɛna, na thɛsɔ, na boka bulosɔ;
66018013	na bi kakɔ, na ni hʋ̃ʋ, na latιkolo, na thɩ̃ɛsɔɔkɛ hɔnι latιkolo ni caar, na thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ n hʋnanι daʋ, na dιvɛ̃, na niin, na mιιn, na thɩ̃ ƴιrɛ hɔnι jɔ, na nʋma, na banaa, na gãgʋʋsɔ, na gãgo hotorosɔ, na deasɔ, narakɛ tibil dolõosɔ.
66018014	Gιrɛra n kɔ fιnι thue gι hʋnɔna fɛr dιphã; dι gιrɛra fɛʋʋkɛ kɔɔ dɔ farnι nũfe thɩ̃ɛ, na thɩ̃ ɓɔna, gι buur farɛ fɛʋ, ga do dayιnanɛ bã.
66018015	Wιrɛ n ƴabananι ga thɩ̃sɔɔle a debi do lɛ̃lɛ dιι do dιιle dɔ nɔɔ, ƴɔɔ wa jιιl maar n fʋlɛ wι ɔɔ 'wãgara, wa khιιrɛ wa-n bιna,
66018016	wa-n sona aa: Gι puurore, gι puure dι kɔ̃tιιnaakɛ n kɔɔ tɔnι kẽkẽ ɓɔna, na kẽkẽ sɛna himə himə, na kẽkẽ sɛna kpakpa, dι gbana dɛ, na bokanaakɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ ka, na lẽbii, dι gbɛbιna dιbara,
66018017	gιdonι lιɛr bιɛl dapaara thakɛ lẽle thɩ̃ jɔjʋɔɔkɛ kʋɛrɛ koo. Dι bato vιrdara fɛʋ, na wιrɛ hanι kpaarɔ lanyʋɔnna, na wιrɛ n dɔnι thɔma bato bιnɔ, na wιrɛ hananι awι nyɛ̃kιɛr thɔ̃ dι wa-n do lanyʋɔnna, wι jιιlɛ ƴɔɔ.
66018018	Mɔ̃ wι yιnι isiir dι ga-n bã ɔɔ hιna, wι-n hulene dι wa-n sona ayɩ: Ʋmɔ̃ɔ dɩ hale a thʋ̃ hona kha dɩ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩkɛ?
66018019	Sa kɛl thɩlãkobe dɩ wa-n dʋna yʋɔsɔ, a khɩɩna dɩ wa-n bɩna, dɩ wa-n hulena ayι: Gι puurore, gι puure dι kɔ̃tιιnana, kɛ ɔɔ lẽle thɩ̃ donι nɔɔ dι wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ hananι bato lanyʋɔnna debiro a do lɛ̃lɛ, gιdonι dapaara lιɛr bιɛl thakɛ a bũburone koo.
66018020	Sι fɛr Thãgbaa dʋɔ na kãkanɛ ɔɔ bũburona, na nɛr tιι phuusɔ, na thɔ̃thɔnasɔ, na Thãgbaa bobonasɔ, gιdonι Thãgba kιιlnaanɛ puureraakɛ a cʋʋ nιnι.
66018021	Dι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuukɛ hananι fãga dιι və̃vĩə kɔɔ gbaar bokaarιkɛ kɔ̃tιnanι a ho nãa tə̃ə, a dʋna lanyʋɔnna sa so: Thakɛra wa dʋna na fãga Babιlɔn dι kɔ̃tɩ̃ιkɛ dι tibil na yιι bã.
66018022	Wa nι salã bιιn na nι wire afι bιnɔ bã; wa nι dakha bel ʋʋn na tutuu ʋʋn afι bιnɔ bã; wa yι nyɛ̃kιɛr thɔ̃ don wo thɔ̃ don afι bιnɔ bã; wa nι dakha jʋ naan afι bιnɔ bã.
66018023	Wa yι lãphã dahιrɛsɔ afι bιnɔ bã; wa nι dakha kũu her na khɛ he tutugore afι bιnɔ bã, gιdonι afι ƴaƴabιdara kɔɔ dor kɔ̃tιna thιιra, afι sidumo thɩ̃ cʋʋ kɔɔ dor nɔɔ dι tibil caar fɛʋ kɔɔ buuro.
66018024	Fɛr Babιlɔn dι bιnɔ wι kɔɔ yι Thãgbaa bobonasɔɔ tɔmɩ̃, na tιι phuusɔɔ tɔmɩ̃, na wιrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ wɩ kɔɔ kʋʋrnɩ thɩɩraakɛɛ tɔmɩ̃.
66019001	A gele pɩ, mɩ nɩrɛ nɔ khena dɩɩ ho tibil jɔjʋɔɔ wi le Thãgbaa dʋɔ, dɩ wa-n so ayɩ: Aleluya, asɩ Thãgba hɩna taarɛ, na i dʋbɩrɛ, na fãga;
66019002	gɩdonɩ ɔɔ kɩɩlsɔ sarrɛ gɩ dor dakha sobɔr. A kɩɩlnanɛ khɛ bɔdɛl kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩlera kɛ n kɔɔ kʋɛanɩ thɩɩ na ɔɔ bɔdɛl cʋʋ. A tiire ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔɔ tɔmɩ̃ hel a lʋʋrʋʋrɛ a tee.
66019003	Dɩ wɩ bir a 'loro balanyɔ wo aa: Aleluya. Dɩ ɔɔ isi bã dɩ ga-n jʋʋn bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ.
66019004	Dɩ kɔ̃tɩna kpelẽ yenã na thɩ̃ ye yenãale gburõku a fʋɔr Thãgbaakɛ tɔɔnɩ fãga too paarra dɩ wa-n sona ayɩ: Amɛn, aleluya.
66019005	Dɩ wire kɔɔ ther fãga too paar ayɩ: Na-n khɩa asɩ Thãgba, nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ dɔnɩ ɔɔ thɔ̃darasɔ, na nɛrɛ fɛʋʋkɛ n maanɛɛnɩ tɩɩ pɔɩ a gbana tɩɩ kɔ̃tɩna.
66019006	Dɩ mɩ kɔɔ nɩrɛ nʋɔ dɩɩ ho tibil jɔjʋɔɔ wi, a hona yɔ jɔjʋɔ n hela, a hona dakha thãgba phɛɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃ɩ, dɩɩ so ayɩ: Aleluya, gιdonι Kɔ̃tιnιkɛ dɔnι asι Thãgba na fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar, ɔr ιrɛna ɔɔ fãgadaar do.
66019007	Sa-n kãkanɛ, sι dɔ daʋ n fʋ sι dakha, sa-n dʋba ɔɔ i, gιdonι Bana bii he wi daan, dι ɔɔ khɛr gbɛbιrɛ pι.
66019008	Thãgba haarɛ hʋɛ dι to kẽkẽ ɓɔ̃ bulo phιphιphιl; kẽkẽ ɓʋ̃ɔ dʋɔn tιι phuusɔɔ fιl sar thɔ̃ɔkɛ wι kɔɔ cʋʋnι.
66019009	Dι thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu so marɛ ayι: Kherene ayɛ: Gι da wɛkɛra Thãgba wenι Bana bii he dιkora. Sι a so marɛ: Gekɛra dɔ Thãgbaa sobɔ thιmιι waa gel.
66019010	Dι mι kɔɔ jire ɔɔ ƴɛra ɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋra, sι a so marɛ ɩ̃ jιɛ hιιn ma-n cʋa' aa, thɔ̃ don ha nι dakha ɩ̃ kha, na ɩ̃ omisɔɔ kha, kɛ fɔrɔnι sobɔrιkɛ Jeju kɔɔ mιιnι; aa, ɩ̃ fʋɔrɛ Thãgba dɔrɔɔm. Jeju sobɔɔkɛ a kɔɔ mιιnι, gɛr n hana Thãgbaa bobonasɔ gιrɛ wι-n mιιnι.
66019011	Agιpι mι yιrɛ Thãgbaa dʋɔ dιι khɛr, dιι do gãgo bulo gι, dι ʋrɛ jʋnɛnι gãgʋʋlera ɔɔ i n dʋɔn Sobɔ cʋʋdaar na Sobɔ bire. Kιιlʋʋkɛ a-n kιιlnι na kɛ̃kɛrɛnɛɛkɛ a-n kɛ̃kɛrɛnι gι sarrɛ.
66019012	Ɔɔ yisɔ hʋrɛ dɔlιnanɛ, sι a subire fãga kpɛra jɔɔ ɔɔ yʋra, dι ire hale a khereraa kɛ tibil na jιnι sι agado ɔrra gaaga.
66019013	A tor kɩ̃kιιnιkɛ mʋanι tɔmιnna, sι ɔɔ i n dʋɔn: Thãgbaa so.
66019014	Dι Thãgbaa dι sɔrasɛ ha sιkaar na gãgo bulona dι wa-n kpaan, a to kẽkẽ bulona phιphιphιl.
66019015	Dι khalgbãakɛ n khɛnι bilə yenyɔ hale a thιι nʋɔra, kɛ a na kʋʋrnanι tibil caar fɛʋ. Ɔr na-n khɛ wι dakha na the gbʋʋl, dι ɔrra na nana be bi nã paar, dι dιvɛ̃ɛkɛ n nɛnanι Thãgba fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daarι nĩkhi khe na ther.
66019016	A hananɛ ire dιι khere ɔɔ kẽkena na ɔɔ huurə ayι: Ɔr dʋɔn Fãgadaar kpιɛ fãgadarara, na Kɔ̃tɩ̃ kpιɛ kɔ̃tιnana.
66019017	Dι mι yιrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bιɛl dι jιιl wirera sa hulẽ dιι khιιr ka, a so 'lominə fɛʋraakɛ n uboni ƴũ dι wa-n kpaar ayι: Nι ιna a gbɛba pa bιɛl a khɔ Thãgbaa dιko kɔ̃tɩ̃.
66019018	Nι ɩna a khɔ fãgadaraa tomɩ, na sɔrasɛɛ kɔ̃tɩ̃sɔɔ tomɩ, na fãga cʋʋdaraa tomɩ, na gãgʋʋsɔ na wɩrɛ n jʋnɛ wɩnɩɩ tomɩ, na tɩbɩla fɛʋʋ tomɩ, waɩa na dea, tɩɩ mɔlɔ na tɩɩ kɔ̃tɩnasɔ.
66019019	Dɩ mɩ yɩrɛ nʋm, na thɩ fãgadara, na awɩ sɔrasɩsɔ fɛʋ, dɩ wɩ kpa jɛ pa bɩɛl wɩ ke kʋʋr na ʋrɛ jʋnɛnɩ gãgʋʋle wɩ kena dakha ɔɔ sɔrasιsɔ.
66019020	Sι wι kɔɔ fʋrɛ nʋmιle na sõso bobonιle dakha, kɛ n kɔɔ cʋɛnι nɔ kpaa thɩ̃ɛ ɔɔ ƴɛra, kɛ dɔnι gιrɛ a-n kɔɔ gbanι da-n fιιlna wιrɛ kɔɔ 'lɛnι nʋmιlee jẽ, kɛ n gburõkuneni thιɛnaakɛ wι cʋʋnι dιι hʋʋ. Wι gba wɛr yenyɔ fɛʋ na yire a dʋna lireraakɛ dɔnι dɔ haar, ka girbi hanι dι ga-n hɩ̃.
66019021	Sι wιrɛ sɛnι khalgbãakɛ thɛnι gãgo jʋʋndaarιlee nɔra kɔɔ kʋrɛ wι, dι 'lominə fɛʋ kɔɔ hire awι nʋ̃ waa phi.
66020001	Agιpι mι yιrɛ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bιɛl dι the Thãgbaa dʋɔ da-n gbũ, a fʋrɔ thɛrɛ 'lee kõkor lakile na jɔrkɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃ι tə̃ə ɔɔ nyɔ̃kɔɔ.
66020002	Dι a fʋrɛ gbakhookɛ dɔnι si tɩ̃ιlera, kɛ n dɔnι kɔ̃tɛɛbiisɔɔ kɔ̃tɩ̃, kɛ n dɔnι dakha Satã, a lii faa yɛna gbιlanι;
66020003	a dʋnaa a faa le thɛrɛ 'lee kõkorʋra sa kpala pɛr, a kpalana dakha jιιn, dι mɛ̃ a na yι hʋɛ a na-n fιιl tibil caar fɛʋra bã, phaphapha yɛna gbιlanι n ka gι pι. Sι agιpι dɔ wι thʋbʋʋ wι faa bɔɔ gbe.
66020004	Agιpι mι yιrɛ fãga too paarsɔ, dι wιrɛɛkɛ tɔɔrɔnι 'lɛr hʋɛ dι wa-n kιιl kιιlʋ; dι mι yιrɛ tιbιlaa thusɔ, kɛ dɔnι wιrɛ wι kɔɔ kuurni yʋʋ dιι do sobɔrιkɛ wι-n kɔɔ mιιnι Jejura na Thãgbaa thιmιιra dɔ nɔɔ, na wɛkɛ na kɔɔ gburõkuneni nʋmιnaale na thιɛnaakɛ wι kɔɔ cʋʋnι dιι hʋa', kɛ dakha na kɔɔ 'lɛnι jιιn kobera dι nyɔɔna ga, dι wι bire a hana yiresɔ dιι do wɛr kɔɔ dɔ kha fãgadara na Kirisiti yɛna gbιlanιιlera.
66020005	Wɩ̃ khisɔɔkɛ sɛnι na bir na 'lɛ yirə' foo yɛna gbιlanιιle n ka ɓo. Gιrɛ dɔ caca khi ιιrɛ.
66020006	Gι da wιrɛraakɛ na hanι caca khi ιιrɛraale, wι dor dakha tιι phuusɔ. Balanyɔ khir na puno na cʋʋ wɩ thɩ̃ɛ bã, sɩ Thãgba na Kirisitii bonɩ jidara wa do, dɩ wɛr na dɔ kha na ɔr fãgadara na cʋʋna yɛna gbɩlanɩɩle.
66020007	A yɛna gbɩlanɩɩle ka pɩ, gɛr wa khɛrrɔ Satã ɔɔ khaɩra na faa.
66020008	Dɩ a na ther a na-n fifilə tibil caarsɔɔkɛ hanɩ thɩ khu paar yenã, kɛ dɔnɩ Gɔɔgɩ na Magɔɔgɩ, a kpa wɩ a jɛ pa bɩɛl kʋʋrra, wa jɔrɛ na ho gbalãkothɩn lanyɔ̃ nʋɔra.
66020009	Wɩ ɩɩrɛ a gba thɩɩra a dii tɩɩ phuusɔɔ jɛ pa, na dɩɩkɛ Thãgba nanɩ. Sɩ dɔɔ ther Thãgbaa dʋɔ a thii wi.
66020010	Dɩ Satãalera n kɔɔ fɩlɛ wɩnɩ, wɩ dʋnaanɛ dɩphã a faa lireraakɛ dɔnɩ dɔ haar na girbi, ka nʋmɩle hanɩ na sõso bobonɩle, liir wa-n 'wãga dɩwɩlʋ na dɩtɩnɛ bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ.
66020011	Dι mι kɔɔ yιrɛ fãga too pa bulo tə̃ə na ʋrɛɛkɛ kɔɔ tɔɔrɔnι; dι ɔɔ ƴɛbʋrɔ thιι na ƴũ fuure sa sιι; wa hale bã.
66020012	Le mι yι khe kɔ̃tιna na tιι mɔlɔsɔ, dι wa-n jιιl fãga too pa ƴιɛra, dι sɛbɛ phubire, dι sɛbɛ kpιι hale wo a phubi, kɛ dɔnι yi sɛbɛ; dι Thãgba kιιlnanɛ khe mɔ̃ a yιɛnι dιι khere sɛbɛraalera mɔ̃ awι thɔ̃ hanι.
66020013	Dι lanyʋɔn 'laarɛ kheekɛ haaraanι, dι khir na khĩdi dιι 'laa kheekɛ hanι awι pa dakha, dι Thãgba kιιlnanɛ kheele fɛʋ bιɛlbιɛl mɔ̃kɛ awι thɔ̃sɔ hanι.
66020014	Dι wι gbaar khir na khĩdi dιι a dʋna faa lireraakɛ dɔnι dɔ haar. Lireele dɔnι dɔ haar gɛr dʋɔn balanyɔ khir.
66020015	Dι ʋrɛ ɔɔ i na kherenι yi sɛbɛra ga, wι dʋnaanɛ faa lireraakɛ dɔnι dɔ haar.
66021001	Dι mι kɔɔ yιrɛ ƴũ phaa na thι phaa, gιdonι caca ƴũukɛ na caca thιιkɛ kɔɔ phor ka, dι lanyʋɔn dakha na hale bã.
66021002	Dι ĩ yι dι phuukɛ dɔnι Jerujalɛm phaa dιι the Thãgbaa pa dι ga-n gbũ, a gbɛbιrι pι a ho khɛ biireekɛ gbɛbanι pι ɔɔ ko n kpaa.
66021003	Dι mι kɔɔ nιrɛ nɔ khιιr dιι the fãga too paar a so ayι: Hιnɛ, Thãgbaa cɔ pa ha kha na tιbιla dιphã, dι ɔr na-n tɔɔ kha na wɛr. Wɛr na dɔ ɔɔ too dι Thãgbaa thɛthɛra na haan kha na wɛr.
66021004	Ɔr na pιιnɛ yilẽbe fɛʋ awι yirə. Khir na hale bã, benιɛ na hale bã, khιιrɛ na hale bã, nιwɛ na hale bã, gιdonι caca thĩɛ phor ka.
66021005	Dι ʋrɛɛkɛ tɔɔnι fãga too paar sor ayι: Hιnɛ, mι cʋʋrɛ thɩ̃ɛ fɛʋ dιι do daphaa. Dι a so marɛ ayι: Khera gιdonι sorιkɛra sobɔr gι waa gel, a do thιmιιrιkɛ teananι ha pɛrɛ.
66021006	Dι a so marɛ wo ayι: Gι daan mɛ̃. mɛr dʋɔn Alfa na Omega, kιrʋ dʋɔn fʋ paar na khu paar. Ʋrɛɛkɛ yɔlkhaa fʋnι, ma haarɛ yi yɔ bu ka nyʋɔn khaar da yɔ;
66021007	gɛr dɔ gιrɛ ʋrɛ kəəneni na 'lɛnι, dι ma dor ɔɔ Thãgba a do ι bikuun.
66021008	Sι ado wιrɛ na hananι 'laraa gι, na ha pɛ 'leedara, na khaakhaardara, na tιι kɔ, na bɔdɛl cʋʋdara, na dɔdɔɔdara, na thɩl je, na sõsodara fɛʋ, awι pa na dɔ lireekɛ dɔnι dɔ haar na girbi, gɛr dɔ balanyɔ khir.
66021009	Agɩpɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu bɩɛl thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu makonyɔraakɛ fʋrɔnɛnɩ bilẽse makonyɔɔkɛ henəni pɩpɩɩ thɩlkena makonyɔ pɔr, a so mar ayɩ: Ɩna kɛ, ma nɩ farɛ khɛrɩkɛ dɔnɩ Bana bii khɛr.
66021010	Dɩɩ do Thu Phuu gɩ, a gba mɩ jʋʋnna gɔ̃gɔ̃ kɔ̃tɩɩnaakɛ gbaanɔnɩ, a nɩ mar dɩ phuukɛ dɔnɩ Jerujalɛm, kɛ thɛnɩ Thãgbaa pa ƴũ a gbũ,
66021011	kɛ Thãgbaa i dʋbɩ donɩ nɔɔ dɩ ga-n carbara. Ɔɔ carã pa n hʋrɛ kha na bokanaakɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ, gɩ hor jasɩpɩ bokaarɩkɛ n hɩlanɩ hɩɩn khaa.
66021012	Go kɔ̃tɩ̃ gbãa diire dɩɩrara, kɛ hananɩ lõfonʋɔ yʋɔr yenyɔ, dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu yʋɔr yenyɔ hale lõfonʋɔ yʋɔr yenyɔrara, dɩ Ɩjɩrayɛl bɩsanaa ca yʋɔr yenyɔɔ i hale a khere lõfonʋɔsɔrara.
66021013	Wi phã paar lõfonʋɔ yẽther; ka wire n phanɩ dɩ pɛ nyɔ̃bɔɔ lõfonʋɔ yẽther; ka wire n phanɩ dɩ pɛ nyɔ̃bɩlã lõfonʋɔ yẽther; gananɔ lõfonʋɔ yẽther.
66021014	Dɩ dɩɩlee gora dɛɛnɛ go kpɛɛrɛ yʋɔr yenyɔra, ka Bana bii thɔ̃thɔna yʋɔr yenyɔɔ i kherenɩ.
66021015	Ʋrɛɛkɛ n mɩana mɩnɩ a fʋrɔrɛ jʋmũu, dɩɩ do thɩ̃ mɩɛdaa sa do dɛ haar, kɛ a na mɩɛnanɩ dɩɩlera, na ɔɔ lõfonɔsɔ, na ɔɔ go.
66021016	Mɔ̃ dɩɩra mɩnɩ ʋ̃ dɩ gãgã mãkhananɛ ʋ̃ dɩ gãgã phɛrɛ; mɔ̃ a gbaannɩ na mɔ̃ a pɩɛrnɩ gɩ mãkharɛ. Dɩ a mɩɛrɛ dɩɩra na jʋmuunə, dɩ gbãʋ thɔɔrɛ kilə gbɩlanɩ yenyɔ na taanyɔ. Gbãʋ, na pɛʋ, na jʋʋnɛ mãkharɛ wɛrɛ.
66021017	A mɩɛrɛ gʋʋ dɩɩ thɔɔ mɛtɛrɛ kpalãther yenã; mɩɛdaakɛ tibil n mɩɛnanɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule mɩɛna.
66021018	Gʋʋra mɩrɛ na jasɩpɩ bokana, dɩ dɛ haar dɩɩra mɩna dɩɩ ho hɩɩn haar.
66021019	Dɩɩlee go kpɛɛsɔra bokanaakɛ khiinoni the nʋɔ ka gɩ kɔɔ gbɛbɩna: Caca go kpɛɛrɛ jasɩpɩ bokana gɩ, balanyɔdaa do safɩɩr bokana, balãtherdaa do agatɩ bokana, balanãdaa do emərodi bokana,
66021020	balamɔɩdaa do onɩsɩ bokana, maadõdaa do sardʋan bokana, makonyɔdaa do kirijoliti bokana, makõtherdaa do beril bokana, yʋɔr phe bidaa do topajɩ bokana, yʋɔrdaa do kirijopɩrasɩ bokana, yʋɔr bɩɛldaa do turkʋajɩ bokana, yʋɔr yenyɔdaa do amɛtɩsɩtɩ bokana.
66021021	Lõfonʋɔ yʋɔr yenyɔɔlera dor lẽbii yʋɔr yenyɔ. Ʋ lõfonɔ do lẽbu bɩɛl, ʋ do lẽbu bɩɛl; sɩ dɩɩlee kʋlã hʋ dɛ haarra gɩ do koo, a ho hɩɩnʋ cacaca.
66021022	Sɩ ma yɩ Thãgbaa cɔ dɩɩraalera ga, gɩdonɩ Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgba fãga fɛʋʋ hɩ̃daar ɔr na Bana bii dɔ Thãgbaa cɔ mɛ̃.
66021023	Dɩɩra na hana wiree ƴaal dɩ por gɩ gɩ hɩrɛnɛna', gɩdonɩ Thãgbaa carbara hɩrɛnɛɛ, dɩ Bana bii do dakha ɔɔ lãphã.
66021024	Dι ɔɔ dahιrɛrara tibil caar fɛʋ na-n ιιr, dι fãgadara thιιraakɛ na gbaar awι nyɔ̃kor bɔ a na pɔnanaa.
66021025	Gιdonι dιtιnɛ na hala', ɔɔ losɔ na hana khaanɛ dιwιlʋla ga.
66021026	Tibil caar fɛʋ na gbaar awι nyɔ̃kor bɔ na cʋʋr a na pɔnanaa.
66021027	Thɩ̃ bɩɛlɩkɛrakɛ dɔnɩ thɩ̃ bise na lõ la', na tɩbɩlaakɛ n cʋɛnɩ kpɔ̃kpɔrɔ̃ thɩ̃ɛ na wɩrɛ n kureni sɔ̃sɔ na lõ la'; wɩrɛ dɩbara awɩ i kherenɩ yi sɛbɛraakɛ dɔnɩ Bana biida, wɛr na lona.
66022001	Dɩ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuule kɔɔ nɩ marɛ mɩɩr yɔ yire wɩwɩwɩl, kɛ n carbaranɛnɩ a ho hɩɩnʋ, a the Thãgba na Bana bii fãga too para,
66022002	dɩ ga-n cel dɩɩlee kʋlã hʋ thɩ̃thιɩn. Dɩ mɩɩr gɛla yenyɔraale thɩr yire hale phonɩ dɩ ga-n se nyẽbe yʋɔr yenyɔ yɛ bɩɛlla, pora pora gɩ-n se, dɩ ɔɔ fa dor thɩɩ tibil caarra.
66022003	Sʋɔn na hale bã. Thãgba na Bana bii fãga too pa na haan dɩɩraalera, dɩ ɔɔ thɔ̃dara na-n dʋʋraarɛ fɔfʋɔr thɔma,
66022004	wa yɩrɛ ɔɔ ƴɛbi, dɩ ɔɔ i na hale awɩ kobisɔra.
66022005	Dɩtɩnɛ na hale bã, dɩ tibil na hana lãphã ƴaalɛ dɩ wiree dahɩrɛ ƴaal gɩ bã, gɩdonɩ Thãgbaakɛ dɔnɩ Kɔ̃tɩn na-n hɩrɛnɛ wɩ; wa dor fãgadara bɔɔ fɛʋ waa khorr vʋ̃ʋ.
66022006	Dɩ a so marɛ ayɩ: Thɩmɩasɔɔkɛra, sobɔr gɩ waa gel, a do thɩmɩaakɛ teananɩ ha pɛrɛ. Kɔ̃tɩnɩkɛ dɔnɩ Thãgbaakɛ n 'laanɛnɩ ɔɔ Thu bobonasɔra, ɔr thɔna ɔɔ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu a nɛna ɔɔ thɔ̃daarsɔ thɩ̃ɛɛkɛ na dananɩ kɔrɔ.
66022007	Hɩnɛ, ma ɩnɛ kɔrɔ. Gɩ da ʋrɛraakɛ n cʋɛnɩ gɩrɛ Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ hanɩ sɛbɛraakɛ sonɩ.
66022008	Mɛr Jã kɔɔ nɩɛnɛ ga thɩ̃ɩkɛra a yɩna gɩ. Dɩ ɔbɔɔkɛ mɩ nɩɛnɩ pɩ a yɩna gɩ, mɩ kɔɔ jire thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thuulee ƴɛra kɛ n nɛ marnɩ ga thɩ̃sɔɔlera ɩ̃ fʋɔrʋʋra.
66022009	Sɩ a so marɛ ayɩ, ɩ̃ jɩɛ hɩɩn ma-n cʋa' aa, thɔ̃ don ha nɩ dakha ɩ̃ kha, na ɩ̃ omisɔɔkɛ dɔnɩ bobonaa kha, na wɩrɛ n cʋɛnɩ gɩrɛ sɛbɛɛkɛ sonɩ aa, ɩ̃ fʋɔrɛ Thãgba dɔrɔɔm.
66022010	Dɩ a so marɛ ayɩ: Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ hanɩ sɛbɛraakɛ, fa-n kpala na jɩɩna', gɩdonɩ bɔɔ n daan.
66022011	Tibilikɛ gõgolonenɩ, a na-n jalana ɔɔ gõgolona; dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ biseneni, a na-n jalana ɔɔ bisera; tɩɩ sarʋ dakha na-n jalana ɔɔ fɩl sarra; dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ phonɩ a na jalana ɔɔ phurə.
66022012	Hɩnɛ, ma ɩnɛ kɔrɔ, dɩ mɩ hananɛ khaardaa a na lɩmɩ tɩbɩla fɛʋ bɩɛlbɩɛl mɔ̃kɛ ntɛɛ thɩ̃ cʋʋ hanɩ.
66022013	Mɛr dʋɔn Alfa na Omega, kɩrʋ dʋɔn cacadaar na pɩpɩɩdaar, fʋ paar na khu paar.
66022014	Gɩ da wɛkɛra n cɔcɔɔnɛnɩ awɩ kẽkẽ, mɛ̃ wa hana hʋɛ a na kho thɩr yiree bi, a na lõ dakha na dɩɩlee lõfonɔ.
66022015	Sɩ bena, na sidumodara, na bɔdɛla, na tɩɩ kɔ, na thɩl je, na wɩrɛ sõso kuure n danɩ haarra dɩ wa-n kuur sɔ̃sɔ, wele fɛʋ na hale dɩ bɩnɔa'.
66022016	Mɛr Jeju, mɛr thɔna ɩ̃ thɔ̃thɔ̃daar thu a mɩa ga thɩmɩɩsɔɔkɛra a hana we gbɛbɩdara. Mɛr dʋɔn Davɩdɩɩ ca, ɔɔ bi məl ha mɩ, dɩ ɩ̃ dona duur ƴepələ̃bireekɛ n caranɛnɩ.
66022017	Dɩ Thu Phuu na Bana bii khɛr dee ayɩ: Ɩna. Ʋrɛɛkɛ nɩɛnɛnɩ dɔ a dee dakha ayɩ: Ɩna. Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ yɔlkhaa fʋnɩ a pɔ, na ʋrɛ n ƴaalɛnɩ yɔ yire a pɔ gba khaar.
66022018	Sɩ mɩ-n kpãkpaanɛ tibil wo tibilləəkɛ n nɩɛnɛnɩ Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩkɛ hanɩ sɛbɛraakɛ ayɩ: A ntɛ gba dɩkha a ɓaan, Thãgba na gbaar thɩlkenaakɛ kheranɩ kɩɛr sɛbɛraakɛ a na pɩɛraa.
66022019	A ntɛ tiro dɩkha Thãgbaa bobonɩ thɩmɩɩraakɛ hanɩ sɛbɛraakɛ, Thãgba na tire ɔɔda dakha thɩr yirera na dɩ phuurəəkɛ kheranɩ kɩɛr sɛbɛraakɛ.
66022020	Dɩ ʋrɛɛkɛ gbaannɩ thɩmɩaakɛ da-n mɩɩ dɩɩ do sobɔr gɩ ayɩwɔɔ aa: Ɔɔ, ma ɩnɛ kɔrɔ. Amɛn, ɩna Jeju Kɔ̃tɩn.
66022021	Jeju Kɔ̃tιn na-n jɛ nɛrɛ fɛʋ bʋɔra.
